Vāgbhaṭa Aṣṭāṅgahṛdayasūtra

sūtrasthāna
rāgādi-rogān satatānuṣaktān a-śeṣa-kāya-prasṛtān a-śeṣān ।
autsukya-mohā-rati-dāñ jaghāna yo a-pūrva-vaidyāya namo astu tasmai ।।

āyuḥ-kāmayamānena dharmārtha-sukha-sādhanam ।
āyur-vedopadeśeṣu vidheyaḥ param ādaraḥ ।।

brahmā smṛtvāyuṣo vedaṃ prajāpatim ajigrahat ।
so aśvinau tau sahasrākṣaṃ so atri-putrādikān munīn ।।

te agniveśādikāṃs te tu pṛthak tantrāṇi tenire ।
tebhyo ati-viprakīrṇebhyaḥ prāyaḥ sāra-taroccayaḥ ।।

kriyate aṣṭāṅga-hṛdayaṃ nāti-saṃkṣepa-vistaram ।
kāya-bāla-grahordhvāṅga-śalya-daṃṣṭrā-jarā-vṛṣān ।।

āti-saṃkṣipta-vistṛtam
aṣṭāv aṅgāni tasyāhuś cikitsā yeṣu saṃśritā ।
vāyuḥ pittaṃ kaphaś ceti trayo doṣāḥ samāsataḥ ।।

vikṛtā-vikṛtā dehaṃ ghnanti te vartayanti ca ।
te vyāpino api hṛn-nābhyor adho-madhyordhva-saṃśrayāḥ ।।

hnanti te vardhayanti ca
vayo-'ho-rātri-bhuktānāṃ te anta-madhyādi-gāḥ kramāt ।
tair bhaved viṣamas tīkṣṇo mandaś cāgniḥ samaiḥ samaḥ ।।

koṣṭhaḥ krūro mṛdur madhyo madhyaḥ syāt taiḥ samair api ।
śukrārtava-sthair janmādau viṣeṇeva viṣa-krimeḥ ।।

taiś ca tisraḥ prakṛtayo hīna-madhyottamāḥ pṛthak ।
sama-dhātuḥ samastāsu śreṣṭhā nindyā dvi-doṣa-jāḥ ।।

ama-dhātuḥ samais tāsu
tatra rūkṣo laghuḥ śītaḥ kharaḥ sūkṣmaś calo anilaḥ ।
pittaṃ sa-sneha-tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ laghu visraṃ saraṃ dravam ।।

snigdhaḥ śīto gurur mandaḥ ślakṣṇo mṛtsnaḥ sthiraḥ kaphaḥ ।
saṃsargaḥ saṃnipātaś ca tad-dvi-tri-kṣaya-kopataḥ ।।

rasāsṛṅ-māṃsa-medo-'sthi-majja-śukrāṇi dhātavaḥ ।
sapta dūṣyā malā mūtra-śakṛt-svedādayo api ca ।।

vṛddhiḥ samānaiḥ sarveṣāṃ viparītair viparyayaḥ ।
rasāḥ svādv-amla-lavaṇa-tiktoṣaṇa-kaṣāyakāḥ ।।

ṣaḍ dravyam āśritās te ca yathā-pūrvaṃ balāvahāḥ ।
tatrādyā mārutaṃ ghnanti trayas tiktādayaḥ kapham ।।

kaṣāya-tikta-madhurāḥ pittam anye tu kurvate ।
śamanaṃ kopanaṃ svastha-hitaṃ dravyam iti tri-dhā ।।

uṣṇa-śīta-guṇotkarṣāt tatra vīryaṃ dvi-dhā smṛtam ।
tri-dhā vipāko dravyasya svādv-amla-kaṭukātmakaḥ ।।

guru-manda-hima-snigdha-ślakṣṇa-sāndra-mṛdu-sthirāḥ ।
guṇāḥ sa-sūkṣma-viśadā viṃśatiḥ sa-viparyayāḥ ।।

kālārtha-karmaṇāṃ yogo hīna-mithyāti-mātrakaḥ ।
samyag-yogaś ca vijñeyo rogārogyaika-kāraṇam ।।

rogas tu doṣa-vaiṣamyaṃ doṣa-sāmyam a-roga-tā ।
nijāgantu-vibhāgena tatra rogā dvi-dhā smṛtāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ kāya-mano-bhedād adhiṣṭhānam api dvi-dhā ।
rajas tamaś ca manaso dvau ca doṣāv udāhṛtau ।।

'tra dvau doṣāv udāhṛtau
darśana-sparśana-praśnaiḥ parīkṣeta ca rogiṇam ।
rogaṃ nidāna-prāg-rūpa-lakṣaṇopaśayāptibhiḥ ।।

aṃparīkṣeta rogiṇam arīkṣetātha rogiṇam
bhūmi-deha-prabhedena deśam āhur iha dvi-dhā ।
jāṅgalaṃ vāta-bhūyiṣṭham anūpaṃ tu kapholbaṇam ।।

sādhāraṇaṃ sama-malaṃ tri-dhā bhū-deśam ādiśet ।
kṣaṇādir vyādhy-avasthā ca kālo bheṣaja-yoga-kṛt ।।

śodhanaṃ śamanaṃ ceti samāsād auṣadhaṃ dvi-dhā ।
śarīra-jānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ krameṇa paramauṣadham ।।

vastir vireko vamanaṃ tathā tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu ।
dhī-dhairyātmādi-vijñānaṃ mano-doṣauṣadhaṃ param ।।

bhiṣag dravyāṇy upasthātā rogī pāda-catuṣṭayam ।
cikitsitasya nirdiṣṭaṃ praty-ekaṃ tac catur-guṇam ।।

dakṣas tīrthātta-śāstrārtho dṛṣṭa-karmā śucir bhiṣak ।
bahu-kalpaṃ bahu-guṇaṃ saṃpannaṃ yogyam auṣadham ।।

anuraktaḥ śucir dakṣo buddhi-mān paricārakaḥ ।
āḍhyo rogī bhiṣag-vaśyo jñāpakaḥ sat-tva-vān api ।।

sādhyo a-sādhya iti vyādhir dvi-dhā tau tu punar dvi-dhā ।
su-sādhyaḥ kṛcchra-sādhyaś ca yāpyo yaś cān-upakramaḥ ।।

sarvauṣadha-kṣame dehe yūnaḥ puṃso jitātmanaḥ ।
a-marma-go alpa-hetv-agra-rūpa-rūpo an-upadravaḥ ।।

a-tulya-dūṣya-deśartu-prakṛtiḥ pāda-saṃpadi ।
graheṣv anu-guṇeṣv eka-doṣa-mārgo navaḥ sukhaḥ ।।

śastrādi-sādhanaḥ kṛcchraḥ saṃkare ca tato gadaḥ ।
śeṣa-tvād āyuṣo yāpyaḥ pathyābhyāsād viparyaye ।।

an-upakrama eva syāt sthito aty-anta-viparyaye ।
autsukya-mohā-rati-kṛd dṛṣṭa-riṣṭo akṣa-nāśanaḥ ।।

tyajed ārtaṃ bhiṣag-bhūpair dviṣṭaṃ teṣāṃ dviṣaṃ dviṣam ।
hīnopakaraṇaṃ vyagram a-vidheyaṃ gatāyuṣam ।।

caṇḍaṃ śokāturaṃ bhīruṃ kṛta-ghnaṃ vaidya-māninam ।
tantrasyāsya paraṃ cāto vakṣyate adhyāya-saṃgrahaḥ ।।

āyuṣ-kāma-dinartv-īhā-rogān-utpādana-dravāḥ ।
anna-jñānānna-saṃrakṣā-mātrā-dravya-rasāśrayāḥ ।।

doṣādi-jñāna-tad-bheda-tac-cikitsā-dvy-upakramāḥ ।
śuddhy-ādi-snehana-sveda-rekāsthāpana-nāvanam ।।

dhūma-gaṇḍūṣa-dṛk-seka-tṛpti-yantraka-śastrakam ।
sirā-vidhiḥ śalya-vidhiḥ śastra-kṣārāgni-karmikau ।।

irā-vyadhaḥ śalya-vidhiḥ
sūtra-sthānam ime adhyāyās triṃśac chārīram ucyate ।
garbhāvakrānti-tad-vyāpad-aṅga-marma-vibhāgikam ।।

vikṛtir dūta-jaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ nidānaṃ sārvarogikam ।
jvarāsṛk-śvāsa-yakṣmādi-madādy-arśo-'tisāriṇām ।।

mūtrāghāta-pramehāṇāṃ vidradhy-ādy-udarasya ca ।
pāṇḍu-kuṣṭhānilārtānāṃ vātāsrasya ca ṣo-ḍaśa ।।

cikitsitaṃ jvare rakte kāse śvāse ca yakṣmaṇi ।
vamau madātyaye arśaḥsu viṣi dvau dvau ca mūtrite ।।

vidradhau gulma-jaṭhara-pāṇḍu-śopha-visarpiṣu ।
kuṣṭha-śvitrānila-vyādhi-vātāsreṣu cikitsitam ।।

dvā-viṃśatir ime adhyāyāḥ kalpa-siddhir ataḥ param ।
kalpo vamer virekasya tat-siddhir vasti-kalpanā ।।

siddhir vasty-āpadāṃ ṣaṣṭho dravya-kalpo ata uttaram ।
bālopacāre tad-vyādhau tad-grahe dvau ca bhūta-ge ।।

unmāde atha smṛti-bhraṃśe dvau dvau vartmasu saṃdhiṣu ।
dṛk-tamo-liṅga-nāśeṣu trayo dvau dvau ca sarva-ge ।।

karṇa-nāsā-mukha-śiro-vraṇe bhaṅge bhagandare ।
granthy-ādau kṣudra-rogeṣu guhya-roge pṛthag dvayam ।।

viṣe bhujaṅge kīṭeṣu mūṣakeṣu rasāyane ।
catvāriṃśo an-apatyānām adhyāyo bīja-poṣaṇaḥ ।।

dhyāyo bīja-poṣaṇe ity adhyāya-śataṃ viṃśaṃ ṣaḍbhiḥ sthānair udīritam ।।

sūtrasthāna
brāhme muhūrta uttiṣṭhet svastho rakṣārtham āyuṣaḥ ।
śarīra-cintāṃ nirvartya kṛta-śauca-vidhis tataḥ ।।

arka-nyagrodha-khadira-karañja-kakubhādi-jam ।
prātar bhuktvā ca mṛdv-agraṃ kaṣāya-kaṭu-tiktakam ।।

kanīny-agra-sama-sthaulyaṃ praguṇaṃ dvā-daśāṅgulam ।
bhakṣayed danta-pavanaṃ danta-māṃsāny a-bādhayan ।।

hakṣayed danta-dhavanaṃ
nādyād a-jīrṇa-vamathu-śvāsa-kāsa-jvarārditī ।
tṛṣṇāsya-pāka-hṛn-netra-śiraḥ-karṇāmayī ca tat ।।

sauvīram añjanaṃ nityaṃ hitam akṣṇos tato bhajet ।
cakṣus tejo-mayaṃ tasya viśeṣāc chleṣmato bhayam ।।

iśeṣāc chleṣmaṇo bhayam
bhukta-vāṃś ca śiraḥ-snātaḥ śrāntaḥ chardana-nāvanaiḥ ।
rātrau jāgaritaś cāpi nāñjyāj jvarita eva ca ।।

yojayet sapta-rātre asmāt srāvaṇārthaṃ rasāñjanam ।
tato nāvana-gaṇḍūṣa-dhūma-tāmbūla-bhāg bhavet ।।

rāvaṇārthe rasāñjanam
tāmbūlaṃ kṣata-pittāsra-rūkṣotkupita-cakṣuṣām ।
viṣa-mūrchā-madārtānām a-pathyaṃ śoṣiṇām api ।।

abhyaṅgam ācaren nityaṃ sa jarā-śrama-vāta-hā ।
dṛṣṭi-prasāda-puṣṭy-āyuḥ-svapna-su-tvak-tva-dārḍhya-kṛt ।।

śiraḥ-śravaṇa-pādeṣu taṃ viśeṣeṇa śīlayet ।
varjyo abhyaṅgaḥ kapha-grasta-kṛta-saṃśuddhy-a-jīrṇibhiḥ ।।

lāghavaṃ karma-sāmarthyaṃ dīpto agnir medasaḥ kṣayaḥ ।
vibhakta-ghana-gātra-tvaṃ vyāyāmād upajāyate ।।

vāta-pittāmayī bālo vṛddho a-jīrṇo ca taṃ tyajet ।
ardha-śaktyā niṣevyas tu balibhiḥ snigdha-bhojibhiḥ ।।

śīta-kāle vasante ca mandam eva tato anya-dā ।
taṃ kṛtvānu-sukhaṃ dehaṃ mardayec ca samantataḥ ।।

tṛṣṇā kṣayaḥ pratamako rakta-pittaṃ śramaḥ klamaḥ ।
ati-vyāyāmataḥ kāso jvaraś chardiś ca jāyate ।।

vyāyāma-jāgarādhva-strī-hāsya-bhāṣyādi-sāhasam ।
gajaṃ siṃha ivākarṣan bhajann ati vinaśyati ।।

hajan yato ati naśyati
udvartanaṃ kapha-haraṃ medasaḥ pravilāyanam ।
sthirī-karaṇam aṅgānāṃ tvak-prasāda-karaṃ param ।।

dīpanaṃ vṛṣyam āyuṣyaṃ snānam ūrjā-bala-pradam ।
kaṇḍū-mala-śrama-sveda-tandrā-tṛḍ-dāha-pāpma-jit ।।

nānam ojo-bala-pradam
uṣṇāmbunādhaḥ-kāyasya pariṣeko balāvahaḥ ।
tenaiva tūttamāṅgasya bala-hṛt-keśa-cakṣuṣām ।।

enaiva cottamāṅgasya a eva cottamāṅgasya a eva 
tūttamāṅgasya
snānam ardita-netrāsya-karṇa-rogātisāriṣu ।
ādhmāna-pīnasā-jīrṇa-bhukta-vatsu ca garhitam ।।

jīrṇe hitaṃ mitaṃ cādyān na vegān īrayed balāt ।
na vegito anya-kāryaḥ syān nā-jitvā sādhyam āmayam ।।

sukhārthāḥ sarva-bhūtānāṃ matāḥ sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ ।
sukhaṃ ca na vinā dharmāt tasmād dharma-paro bhavet ।।

bhaktyā kalyāṇa-mitrāṇi sevetetara-dūra-gaḥ ।
hiṃsā-steyān yathā-kāmaṃ paiśunyaṃ paruṣān-ṛte ।।

saṃbhinnālāpaṃ vyāpādam abhidhyāṃ dṛg-viparyayam ।
pāpaṃ karmeti daśa-dhā kāya-vāṅ-mānasais tyajet ।।

a-vṛtti-vyādhi-śokārtān anuvarteta śaktitaḥ ।
ātma-vat satataṃ paśyed api kīṭa-pipīlikam ।।

arcayed deva-go-vipra-vṛddha-vaidya-nṛpātithīn ।
vi-mukhān nārthinaḥ kuryān nāvamanyeta nākṣipet ।।

upakāra-pradhānaḥ syād apakāra-pare apy arau ।
saṃpad-vipatsv eka-manā hetāv īrṣyet phale na tu ।।

kāle hitaṃ mitaṃ brūyād a-visaṃvādi peśalam ।
pūrvābhibhāṣī su-mukhaḥ su-śīlaḥ karuṇā-mṛduḥ ।।

naikaḥ sukhī na sarva-tra viśrabdho na ca śaṅkitaḥ ।
na kañ-cid ātmanaḥ śatruṃ nātmānaṃ kasya-cid ripum ।।

prakāśayen nāpamānaṃ na ca niḥ-sneha-tāṃ prabhoḥ ।
janasyāśayam ālakṣya yo yathā parituṣyati ।।

rakāśayen nāvamānaṃ
taṃ tathaivānuvarteta parārādhana-paṇḍitaḥ ।
na pīḍayed indriyāṇi na caitāny ati lālayet ।।

tri-varga-śūnyaṃ nārambhaṃ bhajet taṃ cā-virodhayan ।
anuyāyāt prati-padaṃ sarva-dharmeṣu madhyamām ।।

nīca-roma-nakha-śmaśrur nir-malāṅghri-malāyanaḥ ।
snāna-śīlaḥ su-surabhiḥ su-veṣo an-ulbaṇojjvalaḥ ।।

nāna-śīlaḥ sa-surabhiḥ
dhārayet satataṃ ratna-siddha-mantra-mahauṣadhīḥ ।
sātapa-tra-pada-trāṇo vicared yuga-mātra-dṛk ।।

niśi cātyayike kārye daṇḍī maulī sahāya-vān ।
caitya-pūjya-dhvajā-śasta-cchāyā-bhasma-tuṣā-śucīn ।।

nākrāmec charkarā-loṣṭa-bali-snāna-bhuvo na ca ।
nadīṃ taren na bāhubhyāṃ nāgni-skandham abhivrajet ।।

saṃdigdha-nāvaṃ vṛkṣaṃ ca nārohed duṣṭa-yāna-vat ।
nā-saṃvṛta-mukhaḥ kuryāt kṣuti-hāsya-vijṛmbhaṇam ।।

ṣutiṃ hāsyaṃ vijṛmbhaṇam ṣut-hāsyaṃ ca vijṛmbhaṇam
nāsikāṃ na vikuṣṇīyān nā-kasmād vilikhed bhuvam ।
nāṅgaiś ceṣṭeta vi-guṇaṃ nāsītotkaṭakaś ciram ।।

ā-kasmād vilikhen mahīm āsītotkaṭaka-sthitaḥ
deha-vāk-cetasāṃ ceṣṭāḥ prāk śramād vinivartayet ।
nordhva-jānuś ciraṃ tiṣṭhen naktaṃ seveta na drumam ।।

tathā catvara-caityāntaś-catuṣ-patha-surālayān ।
sūnāṭavī-śūnya-gṛha-śmaśānāni divāpi na ।।

a-saṃmārjitam ādarśam an-upaskṛta-kāminīm ।
rajasvalāṃ ca nekṣeta sadā prātar a-maṅgalam ।।

sarva-thekṣeta nādityaṃ na bhāraṃ śirasā vahet ।
nekṣeta pratataṃ sūkṣmaṃ dīptā-medhyā-priyāṇi ca ।।

madya-vikraya-saṃdhāna-dānādānāni nācaret ।
puro-vātātapa-rajas-tuṣāra-paruṣānilān ।।

an-ṛjuḥ kṣavathūdgāra-kāsa-svapnānna-maithunam ।
kūla-cchāyāṃ nṛpa-dviṣṭaṃ vyāla-daṃṣṭri-viṣāṇinaḥ ।।

hīnān-āryāti-nipuṇa-sevāṃ vigraham uttamaiḥ ।
saṃdhyāsv abhyavahāra-strī-svapnādhyayana-cintanam ।।

śatru-sattra-gaṇākīrṇa-gaṇikā-paṇikāśanam ।
gātra-vaktra-nakhair vādyaṃ hasta-keśāvadhūnanam ।।

toyāgni-pūjya-madhyena yānaṃ dhūmaṃ śavāśrayam ।
madyāti-saktiṃ viśrambha-svātantrye strīṣu ca tyajet ।।

ācāryaḥ sarva-ceṣṭāsu loka eva hi dhī-mataḥ ।
anukuryāt tam evāto laukike arthe parīkṣakaḥ ।।

ārdra-saṃtāna-tā tyāgaḥ kāya-vāk-cetasāṃ damaḥ ।
svārtha-buddhiḥ parārtheṣu paryāptam iti sad-vratam ।।

naktan-dināni me yānti katham-bhūtasya saṃprati ।
duḥkha-bhāṅ na bhavaty evaṃ nityaṃ saṃnihita-smṛtiḥ ।।

evaṃ kṛtsna-dinaṃ nītvā rātrau yāme gṛhe gate ।
devān ṛṣīn gurūn smṛtvā tataḥ śayanam ācaret ।।

ātrer yāme gate sati
ity ācāraḥ samāsena yaṃ prāpnoti samācaran ।
āyur ārogyam aiśvaryaṃ yaśo lokāṃś ca śāśvatān ।।

sūtrasthāna
māsair dvi-saṃkhyair māghādyaiḥ kramāt ṣaḍ ṛtavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
śiśiro atha vasantaś ca grīṣmo varṣā-śarad-dhimāḥ ।।

śiśirādyās tribhis tais tu vidyād ayanam uttaram ।
ādānaṃ ca tad ādatte nṛṇāṃ prati-dinaṃ balam ।।

tasmin hy aty-artha-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-rūkṣā mārga-sva-bhāvataḥ ।
āditya-pavanāḥ saumyān kṣapayanti guṇān bhuvaḥ ।।

tiktaḥ kaṣāyaḥ kaṭuko balino atra rasāḥ kramāt ।
tasmād ādānam āgneyam ṛtavo dakṣiṇāyanam ।।

varṣādayo visargaś ca yad balaṃ visṛjaty ayam ।
saumya-tvād atra somo hi bala-vān hīyate raviḥ ।।

megha-vṛṣṭy-anilaiḥ śītaiḥ śānta-tāpe mahī-tale ।
snigdhāś cehāmla-lavaṇa-madhurā balino rasāḥ ।।

śīte agryaṃ vṛṣṭi-gharme alpaṃ balaṃ madhyaṃ tu śeṣayoḥ ।
balinaḥ śīta-saṃrodhād dhemante prabalo analaḥ ।।

bhavaty alpendhano dhātūn sa paced vāyuneritaḥ ।
ato hime asmin seveta svādv-amla-lavaṇān rasān ।।

dairghyān niśānām etarhi prātar eva bubhukṣitaḥ ।
avaśya-kāryaṃ saṃbhāvya yathoktaṃ śīlayed anu ।।

vāta-ghna-tailair abhyaṅgaṃ mūrdhni tailaṃ vimardanam ।
niyuddhaṃ kuśalaiḥ sārdhaṃ pādāghātaṃ ca yuktitaḥ ।।

ūrdha-tailaṃ vimardanam
kaṣāyāpahṛta-snehas tataḥ snāto yathā-vidhi ।
kuṅkumena sa-darpeṇa pradigdho aguru-dhūpitaḥ ।।

rasān snigdhān palaṃ puṣṭaṃ gauḍam accha-surāṃ surām ।
godhūma-piṣṭa-māṣekṣu-kṣīrottha-vikṛtīḥ śubhāḥ ।।

navam annaṃ vasāṃ tailaṃ śauca-kārye sukhodakam ।
prāvārājina-kauśeya-praveṇī-kaucavāstṛtam ।।

-praveṇī-kuthakāstṛtam
uṣṇa-sva-bhāvair laghubhiḥ prāvṛtaḥ śayanaṃ bhajet ।
yuktyārka-kiraṇān svedaṃ pāda-trāṇaṃ ca sarva-dā ।।

pīvaroru-stana-śroṇyaḥ sa-madāḥ pramadāḥ priyāḥ ।
haranti śītam uṣṇāṅgyo dhūpa-kuṅkuma-yauvanaiḥ ।।

aṅgāra-tāpa-saṃtapta-garbha-bhū-veśma-cāriṇaḥ ।
śīta-pāruṣya-janito na doṣo jātu jāyate ।।

ayam eva vidhiḥ kāryaḥ śiśire api viśeṣataḥ ।
tadā hi śītam adhikaṃ raukṣyaṃ cādāna-kāla-jam ।।

kaphaś cito hi śiśire vasante arkāṃśu-tāpitaḥ ।
hatvāgniṃ kurute rogān atas taṃ tvarayā tyajet ।।

tīkṣṇair vamana-nasyādyair laghu-rūkṣaiś ca bhojanaiḥ ।
vyāyāmodvartanāghātair jitvā śleṣmāṇam ulbaṇam ।।

snāto anuliptaḥ karpūra-candanāguru-kuṅkumaiḥ ।
purāṇa-yava-godhūma-kṣaudra-jāṅgala-śūlya-bhuk ।।

sahakāra-rasonmiśrān āsvādya priyayārpitān ।
priyāsya-saṅga-surabhīn priyā-netrotpalāṅkitān ।।

saumanasya-kṛto hṛdyān vayasyaiḥ sahitaḥ pibet ।
nirgadān āsavāriṣṭa-sīdhu-mārdvīka-mādhavān ।।

śṛṅgaverāmbu sārāmbu madhv-ambu jaladāmbu ca ।
dakṣiṇānila-śīteṣu parito jala-vāhiṣu ।।

adhv-ambu jaladāmbu vā
a-dṛṣṭa-naṣṭa-sūryeṣu maṇi-kuṭṭima-kāntiṣu ।
parapuṣṭa-vighuṣṭeṣu kāma-karmānta-bhūmiṣu ।।

-dṛṣṭā-naṣṭa-sūryeṣu
vicitra-puṣpa-vṛkṣeṣu kānaneṣu su-gandhiṣu ।
goṣṭhī-kathābhiś citrābhir madhyāhnaṃ gamayet sukhī ।।

guru-śīta-divā-svapna-snigdhāmla-madhurāṃs tyajet ।
tīkṣṇāṃśur ati-tīkṣṇāṃśur grīṣme saṃkṣipatīva yat ।।

neham arko ati-tīkṣṇāṃśur
praty-ahaṃ kṣīyate śleṣmā tena vāyuś ca vardhate ।
ato asmin paṭu-kaṭv-amla-vyāyāmārka-karāṃs tyajet ।।

bhajen madhuram evānnaṃ laghu snigdhaṃ himaṃ dravam ।
su-śīta-toya-siktāṅgo lihyāt saktūn sa-śarkarān ।।

madyaṃ na peyaṃ peyaṃ vā sv-alpaṃ su-bahu-vāri vā ।
anya-thā śoṣa-śaithilya-dāha-mohān karoti tat ।।

nya-thā śopha-śaithilya-
kundendu-dhavalaṃ śālim aśnīyāj jāṅgalaiḥ palaiḥ ।
pibed rasaṃ nāti-ghanaṃ rasālāṃ rāga-khāṇḍavau ।।

undendu-dhavalāñ chālīn asālāṃ rāga-khāḍavau 
rasālāṃ rāga-ṣāḍavau
pānakaṃ pañca-sāraṃ vā nava-mṛd-bhājane sthitam ।
moca-coca-dalair yuktaṃ sāmlaṃ mṛn-maya-śuktibhiḥ ।।

ava-mṛd-bhājana-sthitam
pāṭalā-vāsitaṃ cāmbhaḥ sa-karpūraṃ su-śītalam ।
śaśāṅka-kiraṇān bhakṣyān rajanyāṃ bhakṣayan pibet ।।

sa-sitaṃ māhiṣaṃ kṣīraṃ candra-nakṣatra-śītalam ।
abhraṅ-kaṣa-mahā-śāla-tāla-ruddhoṣṇa-raśmiṣu ।।

vaneṣu mādhavī-śliṣṭa-drākṣā-stabaka-śāliṣu ।
su-gandhi-hima-pānīya-sicyamāna-paṭālike ।।

kāyamāne cite cūta-pravāla-phala-lumbibhiḥ ।
kadalī-dala-kalhāra-mṛṇāla-kamalotpalaiḥ ।।

komalaiḥ kalpite talpe hasat-kusuma-pallave ।
madhyan-dine arka-tāpārtaḥ svapyād dhārā-gṛhe atha-vā ।।

pusta-strī-stana-hastāsya-pravṛttośīra-vāriṇi ।
niśā-kara-karākīrṇe saudha-pṛṣṭhe niśāsu ca ।।

āsanā svastha-cittasya candanārdrasya mālinaḥ ।
nivṛtta-kāma-tantrasya su-sūkṣma-tanu-vāsasaḥ ।।

jalārdrās tāla-vṛntāni vistṛtāḥ padminī-puṭāḥ ।
utkṣepāś ca mṛdūtkṣepā jala-varṣi-himānilāḥ ।।

karpūra-mallikā-mālā hārāḥ sa-hari-candanāḥ ।
mano-hara-kalālāpāḥ śiśavaḥ sārikāḥ śukāḥ ।।

mṛṇāla-valayāḥ kāntāḥ protphulla-kamalojjvalāḥ ।
jaṅgamā iva padminyo haranti dayitāḥ klamam ।।

ādāna-glāna-vapuṣām agniḥ sanno api sīdati ।
varṣāsu doṣair duṣyanti te ambu-lambāmbu-de ambare ।।

ādāna-mlāna-vapuṣām
sa-tuṣāreṇa marutā sahasā śītalena ca ।
bhū-bāṣpeṇāmla-pākena malinena ca vāriṇā ।।

vahninaiva ca mandena teṣv ity anyo-'nya-dūṣiṣu ।
bhajet sādhāraṇaṃ sarvam ūṣmaṇas tejanaṃ ca yat ।।

āsthāpanaṃ śuddha-tanur jīrṇaṃ dhānyaṃ rasān kṛtān ।
jāṅgalaṃ piśitaṃ yūṣān madhv-ariṣṭaṃ ciran-tanam ।।

mastu sauvarcalāḍhyaṃ vā pañca-kolāvacūrṇitam ।
divyaṃ kaupaṃ śṛtaṃ cāmbho bhojanaṃ tv ati-dur-dine ।।

astu sauvarcalāḍhyaṃ ca
vyaktāmla-lavaṇa-snehaṃ saṃśuṣkaṃ kṣaudra-val laghu ।
a-pāda-cārī surabhiḥ satataṃ dhūpitāmbaraḥ ।।

harmya-pṛṣṭhe vased bāṣpa-śīta-sīkara-varjite ।
nadī-jaloda-manthāhaḥ-svapnāyāsātapāṃś tyajet ।।

varṣā-śītocitāṅgānāṃ sahasaivārka-raśmibhiḥ ।
taptānāṃ saṃcitaṃ vṛṣṭau pittaṃ śaradi kupyati ।।

taj-jayāya ghṛtaṃ tiktaṃ vireko rakta-mokṣaṇam ।
tiktaṃ svādu kaṣāyaṃ ca kṣudhito annaṃ bhajel laghu ।।

śāli-mudga-sitā-dhātrī-paṭola-madhu-jāṅgalam ।
taptaṃ taptāṃśu-kiraṇaiḥ śītaṃ śītāṃśu-raśmibhiḥ ।।

samantād apy aho-rātram agastyodaya-nir-viṣam ।
śuci haṃsodakaṃ nāma nir-malaṃ mala-jij jalam ।।

nābhiṣyandi na vā rūkṣaṃ pānādiṣv amṛtopamam ।
candanośīra-karpūra-muktā-srag-vasanojjvalaḥ ।।

saudheṣu saudha-dhavalāṃ candrikāṃ rajanī-mukhe ।
tuṣāra-kṣāra-sauhitya-dadhi-taila-vasātapān ।।

tīkṣṇa-madya-divā-svapna-puro-vātān parityajet ।
śīte varṣāsu cādyāṃs trīn vasante antyān rasān bhajet ।।

svāduṃ nidāghe śaradi svādu-tikta-kaṣāyakān ।
śarad-vasantayo rūkṣaṃ śītaṃ gharma-ghanāntayoḥ ।।

anna-pānaṃ samāsena viparītam ato anya-dā ।
nityaṃ sarva-rasābhyāsaḥ sva-svādhikyam ṛtāv ṛtau ।।

ṛtvor antyādi-saptāhāv ṛtu-saṃdhir iti smṛtaḥ ।
tatra pūrvo vidhis tyājyaḥ sevanīyo aparaḥ kramāt ।।

ṛtvor antyādi-saptāhād a-sātmya-jā hi rogāḥ syuḥ sahasā tyāga-śīlanāt ।।

sūtrasthāna
vegān na dhārayed vāta-viṇ-mūtra-kṣava-tṛṭ-kṣudhām ।
nidrā-kāsa-śrama-śvāsa-jṛmbhāśru-cchardi-retasām ।।

adho-vātasya rodhena gulmodāvarta-ruk-klamāḥ ।
vāta-mūtra-śakṛt-saṅga-dṛṣṭy-agni-vadha-hṛd-gadāḥ ।।

sneha-sveda-vidhis tatra vartayo bhojanāni ca ।
pānāni vastayaś caiva śastaṃ vātānulomanam ।।

śakṛtaḥ piṇḍikodveṣṭa-pratiśyāya-śiro-rujaḥ ।
ūrdhva-vāyuḥ parīkarto hṛdayasyoparodhanam ।।

ūrdhvaṃ vāyuḥ parīkarto
mukhena viṭ-pravṛttiś ca pūrvoktāś cāmayāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
aṅga-bhaṅgāśmarī-vasti-meḍhra-vaṅkṣaṇa-vedanāḥ ।।

mūtrasya rodhāt pūrve ca prāyo rogās tad-auṣadham ।
varty-abhyaṅgāvagāhāś ca svedanaṃ vasti-karma ca ।।

anna-pānaṃ ca viḍ-bhedi viḍ-rodhottheṣu yakṣmasu ।
mūtra-jeṣu tu pāne ca prāg-bhaktaṃ śasyate ghṛtam ।।

ūtra-jeṣu ca pānaṃ tu ūtra-jeṣu prayuñjīta arpiṣaś 
cāvapīḍakam
jīrṇāntikaṃ cottamayā mātrayā yojanā-dvayam ।
avapīḍakam etac ca saṃjñitaṃ dhāraṇāt punaḥ ।।

udgārasyā-ruciḥ kampo vibandho hṛdayorasoḥ ।
ādhmāna-kāsa-hidhmāś ca hidhmā-vat tatra bheṣajam ।।

śiro-'rtīndriya-daurbalya-manyā-stambhārditaṃ kṣuteḥ ।
tīkṣṇa-dhūmāñjanāghrāṇa-nāvanārka-vilokanaiḥ ।।

pravartayet kṣutiṃ saktāṃ sneha-svedau ca śīlayet ।
śoṣāṅga-sāda-bādhirya-saṃmoha-bhrama-hṛd-gadāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāyā nigrahāt tatra śītaḥ sarvo vidhir hitaḥ ।
aṅga-bhaṅgā-ruci-glāni-kārśya-śūla-bhramāḥ kṣudhaḥ ।।

-kārśya-śūla-śrama-bhramāḥ
tatra yojyaṃ laghu snigdham uṣṇam alpaṃ ca bhojanam ।
nidrāyā moha-mūrdhākṣi-gauravālasya-jṛmbhikāḥ ।।

aivarṇyaṃ ca kṣudhas tatra nigdhoṣṇaṃ laghu bhojanam
aṅga-mardaś ca tatreṣṭaḥ svapnaḥ saṃvāhanāni ca ।
kāsasya rodhāt tad-vṛddhiḥ śvāsā-ruci-hṛd-āmayāḥ ।।

śoṣo hidhmā ca kāryo atra kāsa-hā su-tarāṃ vidhiḥ ।
gulma-hṛd-roga-saṃmohāḥ śrama-śvāsād vidhāritāt ।।

śrama-śvāsā-vidhāraṇāt
hitaṃ viśramaṇaṃ tatra vāta-ghnaś ca kriyā-kramaḥ ।
jṛmbhāyāḥ kṣava-vad rogāḥ sarvaś cānila-jid vidhiḥ ।।

c jṛmbhāyāḥ kṣuti-vad rogāḥ
pīnasākṣi-śiro-hṛd-ruṅ-manyā-stambhā-ruci-bhramāḥ ।
sa-gulmā bāṣpatas tatra svapno madyaṃ priyāḥ kathāḥ ।।

visarpa-koṭha-kuṣṭhākṣi-kaṇḍū-pāṇḍv-āmaya-jvarāḥ ।
sa-kāsa-śvāsa-hṛl-lāsa-vyaṅga-śvayathavo vameḥ ।।

gaṇḍūṣa-dhūmān-āhārā rūkṣaṃ bhuktvā tad-udvamaḥ ।
vyāyāmaḥ srutir asrasya śastaṃ cātra virecanam ।।

aṇḍūṣa-dhūmān-āhāraṃ aṇḍūṣa-dhūmān-āhārān ūkṣaṃ bhuktvā tad udvamet 
ūkṣān bhuktvā tad udvamet
sa-kṣāra-lavaṇaṃ tailam abhyaṅgārthaṃ ca śasyate ।
śukrāt tat-sravaṇaṃ guhya-vedanā-śvayathu-jvarāḥ ।।

bhyaṅgārthe ca śasyate
hṛd-vyathā-mūtra-saṅgāṅga-bhaṅga-vṛddhy-aśma-ṣaṇḍha-tāḥ ।
tāmra-cūḍa-surā-śāli-vasty-abhyaṅgāvagāhanam ।।

vasti-śuddhi-karaiḥ siddhaṃ bhajet kṣīraṃ priyāḥ striyaḥ ।
tṛṭ-śūlārtaṃ tyajet kṣīṇaṃ viḍ-vamaṃ vega-rodhinam ।।

rogāḥ sarve api jāyante vegodīraṇa-dhāraṇaiḥ ।
nirdiṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ tatra bhūyiṣṭhaṃ ye tu tān prati ।।

tataś cāneka-dhā prāyaḥ pavano yat prakupyati ।
anna-pānauṣadhaṃ tasya yuñjītāto anulomanam ।।

dhārayet tu sadā vegān hitaiṣī pretya ceha ca ।
lobherṣyā-dveṣa-mātsarya-rāgādīnāṃ jitendriyaḥ ।।

yateta ca yathā-kālaṃ malānāṃ śodhanaṃ prati ।
aty-artha-saṃcitās te hi kruddhāḥ syur jīvita-cchidaḥ ।।

doṣāḥ kadā-cit kupyanti jitā laṅghana-pācanaiḥ ।
ye tu saṃśodhanaiḥ śuddhā na teṣāṃ punar-udbhavaḥ ।।

e tu saṃśodhanaiḥ śuddhās eṣāṃ na punar-udbhavaḥca
yathā-kramaṃ yathā-yogam ata ūrdhvaṃ prayojayet ।
rasāyanāni siddhāni vṛṣya-yogāṃś ca kāla-vit ।।

athā-kramaṃ yathā-yogyam
bheṣaja-kṣapite pathyam āhārair bṛṃhaṇaṃ kramāt ।
śāli-ṣaṣṭika-godhūma-mudga-māṃsa-ghṛtādibhiḥ ।।

-mudga-māṃsa-rasādibhiḥ
hṛdya-dīpana-bhaiṣajya-saṃyogād ruci-pakti-daiḥ ।
sābhyaṅgodvartana-snāna-nirūha-sneha-vastibhiḥ ।।

tathā sa labhate śarma sarva-pāvaka-pāṭavam ।
dhī-varṇendriya-vaimalyaṃ vṛṣa-tāṃ dairghyam āyuṣaḥ ।।

ye bhūta-viṣa-vāyv-agni-kṣata-bhaṅgādi-saṃbhavāḥ ।
rāga-dveṣa-bhayādyāś ca te syur āgantavo gadāḥ ।।

āma-krodha-bhāyādyāś
tyāgaḥ prajñāparādhānām indriyopaśamaḥ smṛtiḥ ।
deśa-kālātma-vijñānaṃ sad-vṛttasyānuvartanam ।।

atharva-vihitā śāntiḥ pratikūla-grahārcanam ।
bhūtādya-sparśanopāyo nirdiṣṭaś ca pṛthak pṛthak ।।

an-utpattyai samāsena vidhir eṣa pradarśitaḥ ।
nijāgantu-vikārāṇām utpannānāṃ ca śāntaye ।।

n-utpattau samāsena
śītodbhavaṃ doṣa-cayaṃ vasante viśodhayan grīṣma-jam abhra-kāle ।
ghanātyaye vārṣikam āśu samyak prāpnoti rogān ṛtu-jān na jātu ।।

nityaṃ hitāhāra-vihāra-sevī samīkṣya-kārī viṣayeṣv a-saktaḥ ।
dātā samaḥ satya-paraḥ kṣamā-vān āptopasevī ca bhavaty a-rogaḥ ।।

sūtrasthāna
jīvanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ hṛdyaṃ hlādi buddhi-prabodhanam ।
tanv a-vyakta-rasaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ śītaṃ laghv amṛtopamam ।।

gaṅgāmbu nabhaso bhraṣṭaṃ spṛṣṭaṃ tv arkendu-mārutaiḥ ।
hitā-hita-tve tad bhūyo deśa-kālāv apekṣate ।।

yenābhivṛṣṭam a-malaṃ śāly-annaṃ rājate sthitam ।
a-klinnam a-vi-varṇaṃ ca tat peyaṃ gāṅgam anya-thā ।।

śāly-annaṃ rājata-sthitam -klinnam a-vi-varṇaṃ syāt -klinnam a-vivarṇaṃ vā 
at toyaṃ gāṅgam anya-thā
sāmudraṃ tan na pātavyaṃ māsād āśvayujād vinā ।
aindram ambu su-pātra-stham a-vipannaṃ sadā pibet ।।

tad-a-bhāve ca bhūmi-ṣṭham āntarikṣānukāri yat ।
śuci-pṛthv-asita-śvete deśe arka-pavanāhatam ।।

ad-a-bhāve ca bhūyiṣṭham ad-a-bhāve pibed bhaumam
na pibet paṅka-śaivāla-tṛṇa-parṇāvilāstṛtam ।
sūryendu-pavanā-dṛṣṭam abhivṛṣṭaṃ ghanaṃ guru ।।

phenilaṃ jantu-mat taptaṃ danta-grāhy ati-śaityataḥ ।
an-ārtavaṃ ca yad divyam ārtavaṃ prathamaṃ ca yat ।।

lūtādi-tantu-viṇ-mūtra-viṣa-saṃśleṣa-dūṣitam ।
paścimoda-dhi-gāḥ śīghra-vahā yāś cā-malodakāḥ ।।

pathyāḥ samāsāt tā nadyo viparītās tv ato anya-thā ।
upalāsphālanākṣepa-vicchedaiḥ kheditodakāḥ ।।

athyāḥ samāsato nadyo
himavan-malayodbhūtāḥ pathyās tā eva ca sthirāḥ ।
kṛmi-ślīpada-hṛt-kaṇtha-śiro-rogān prakurvate ।।

prācyāvanty-aparāntotthā dur-nāmāni mahendra-jāḥ ।
udara-ślīpadātaṅkān sahya-vindhyodbhavāḥ punaḥ ।।

ahya-vindhya-bhavāḥ punaḥ
kuṣṭha-pāṇḍu-śiro-rogān doṣa-ghnyaḥ pāriyātra-jāḥ ।
bala-pauruṣa-kāriṇyaḥ sāgarāmbhas tri-doṣa-kṛt ।।

āgarāmbu tri-doṣa-kṛt
āvilaṃ sa-malaṃ nīlaṃ ghanaṃ pītam athāpi ca ।
sa-kṣāraṃ picchilaṃ caiva sāmudraṃ tan nigadyate ।।

vidyāt kūpa-taḍāgādīn jāṅgalānūpa-śailataḥ ।
nāmbu peyam a-śaktyā vā sv-alpam alpāgni-gulmibhiḥ ।।

pāṇḍūdarātisārārśo-grahaṇī-śoṣa-śothibhiḥ ।
ṛte śaran-nidāghābhyāṃ pibet svastho api cālpa-śaḥ ।।

-grahaṇī-doṣa-śothibhiḥ
sama-sthūla-kṛśā bhukta-madhyānta-prathamāmbu-pāḥ ।
śītaṃ madātyaya-glāni-mūrchā-chardi-śrama-bhramān ।।

ama-sthūla-kṛśā bhakta-
tṛṣṇoṣṇa-dāha-pittāsra-viṣāṇy ambu niyacchati ।
dīpanaṃ pācanaṃ kaṇṭhyaṃ laghūṣṇaṃ vasti-śodhanam ।।

ṛṣṇoṣma-dāha-pittāsra-
hidhmādhmānānila-śleṣma-sadyaḥ-śuddhi-nava-jvare ।
kāsāma-pīnasa-śvāsa-pārśva-rukṣu ca śasyate ।।

-sadyaḥ-śuddhe nava-jvare
an-abhiṣyandi laghu ca toyaṃ kvathita-śītalam ।
pitta-yukte hitaṃ doṣe vyuṣitaṃ tat tri-doṣa-kṛt ।।

ūkṣam an-abhiṣyandi aghu kvathita-śītalam 
adhyuṣitaṃ tat tri-doṣa-kṛt
nārikelodakaṃ snigdhaṃ svādu vṛṣyaṃ himaṃ laghu ।
tṛṣṇā-pittānila-haraṃ dīpanaṃ vasti-śodhanam ।।

varṣāsu divya-nādeye paraṃ toye varāvare ।
svādu-pāka-rasaṃ snigdham ojasyaṃ dhātu-vardhanam ।।

vāta-pitta-haraṃ vṛṣyaṃ śleṣmalaṃ guru śītalam ।
prāyaḥ payo atra gavyaṃ tu jīvanīyaṃ rasāyanam ।।

kṣata-kṣīṇa-hitaṃ medhyaṃ balyaṃ stanya-karaṃ saram ।
śrama-bhrama-madā-lakṣmī-śvāsa-kāsāti-tṛṭ-kṣudhaḥ ।।

-śvāsa-kāsārti-tṛṭ-kṣudhaḥ -śvāsa-kāsādhi-tṛṭ-kṣudhaḥ
jīrṇa-jvaraṃ mūtra-kṛcchraṃ rakta-pittaṃ ca nāśayet ।
hitam aty-agny-a-nidrebhyo garīyo māhiṣaṃ himam ।।

alpāmbu-pāna-vyāyāma-kaṭu-tiktāśanair laghu ।
ājaṃ śoṣa-jvara-śvāsa-rakta-pittātisāra-jit ।।

īṣad-rūkṣoṣṇa-lavaṇam auṣṭrākam dīpanaṃ laghu ।
śastaṃ vāta-kaphānāha-kṛmi-śophodarārśasām ।।

mānuṣaṃ vāta-pittāsṛg-abhighātākṣi-roga-jit ।
tarpaṇāścyotanair nasyair a-hṛdyaṃ tūṣṇam āvikam ।।

vāta-vyādhi-haraṃ hidhmā-śvāsa-pitta-kapha-pradam ।
hastinyāḥ sthairya-kṛd bāḍham uṣṇaṃ tv aikaśaphaṃ laghu ।।

śākhā-vāta-haraṃ sāmla-lavaṇaṃ jaḍa-tā-karam ।
payo abhiṣyandi gurv āmaṃ yuktyā śṛtam ato anya-thā ।।
vinā tu vanitā-stanyam āmam eva hitaṃ hi tat ।।
bhaved garīyo ati-śṛtaṃ dhāroṣṇam amṛtopamam ।
amla-pāka-rasaṃ grāhi gurūṣṇaṃ dadhi vāta-jit ।।

medaḥ-śukra-bala-śleṣma-pitta-raktāgni-śopha-kṛt ।
rociṣṇu śastam a-rucau śītake viṣama-jvare ।।

pīnase mūtra-kṛcchre ca rūkṣaṃ tu grahaṇī-gade ।
naivādyān niśi naivoṣṇaṃ vasantoṣṇa-śaratsu na ।।

śarad-grīṣma-vasanteṣu ādyān noṣṇaṃ na rātriṣu
nā-mudga-sūpaṃ nā-kṣaudraṃ tan nā-ghṛta-sitopalam ।
na cān-āmalakaṃ nāpi nityaṃ no mandam anya-thā ।।

jvarāsṛk-pitta-vīsarpa-kuṣṭha-pāṇḍu-bhrama-pradam ।
takraṃ laghu kaṣāyāmlaṃ dīpanaṃ kapha-vāta-jit ।।

śophodarārśo-grahaṇī-doṣa-mūtra-grahā-rucīḥ ।
plīha-gulma-ghṛta-vyāpad-gara-pāṇḍv-āmayāñ jayet ।।

tad-van mastu saraṃ srotaḥ-śodhi viṣṭambha-jil laghu ।
nava-nītaṃ navaṃ vṛṣyaṃ śītaṃ varṇa-balāgni-kṛt ।।

saṃgrāhi vāta-pittāsṛk-kṣayārśo-'rdita-kāsa-jit ।
kṣīrodbhavaṃ tu saṃgrāhi rakta-pittākṣi-roga-jit ।।

śastaṃ dhī-smṛti-medhāgni-balāyuḥ-śukra-cakṣuṣām ।
bāla-vṛddha-prajā-kānti-saukumārya-svarārthinām ।।

kṣata-kṣīṇa-parīsarpa-śastrāgni-glapitātmanām ।
vāta-pitta-viṣonmāda-śoṣā-lakṣmī-jvarāpaham ।।

snehānām uttamaṃ śītaṃ vayasaḥ sthāpanaṃ param ।
sahasra-vīryaṃ vidhibhir ghṛtaṃ karma-sahasra-kṛt ।।

ahasra-vīryaṃ vidhi-vad
madāpasmāra-mūrchāya-śiraḥ-karṇākṣi-yoni-jān ।
purāṇaṃ jayati vyādhīn vraṇa-śodhana-ropaṇam ।।

balyāḥ kilāṭa-pīyūṣa-kūrcikā-moraṇādayaḥ ।
śukra-nidrā-kapha-karā viṣṭambhi-guru-doṣalāḥ ।।

-kūcikā-moraṇādayaḥ
gavye kṣīra-ghṛte śreṣṭhe nindite cāvi-saṃbhave ।
ikṣoḥ saro guruḥ snigdho bṛṃhaṇaḥ kapha-mūtra-kṛt ।।

vṛṣyaḥ śīto asra-pitta-ghnaḥ svādu-pāka-raso rasaḥ ।
so agre sa-lavaṇo danta-pīḍitaḥ śarkarā-samaḥ ।।

mūlāgra-jantu-jagdhādi-pīḍanān mala-saṃkarāt ।
kiñ-cit-kālaṃ vidhṛtyā ca vikṛtiṃ yāti yāntrikaḥ ।।

iñ-cit-kāla-vidhṛtyā ca
vidāhī guru-viṣṭambhī tenāsau tatra pauṇḍrakaḥ ।
śaitya-prasāda-mādhuryair varas tam anu vāṃśikaḥ ।।

urur vidāhī viṣṭambhī
śataparvaka-kāntāra-naipālādyās tataḥ kramāt ।
sa-kṣārāḥ sa-kaṣāyāś ca soṣṇāḥ kiñ-cid-vidāhinaḥ ।।

śātaparvaka-kāntāra- -nepālādyās tataḥ kramāt
phāṇitaṃ gurv abhiṣyandi caya-kṛn mūtra-śodhanam ।
nāti-śleṣma-karo dhautaḥ sṛṣṭa-mūtra-śakṛd guḍaḥ ।।

prabhūta-kṛmi-majjāsṛṅ-medo-māṃsa-kapho aparaḥ ।
hṛdyaḥ purāṇaḥ pathyaś ca navaḥ śleṣmāgni-sāda-kṛt ।।

vṛṣyāḥ kṣīṇa-kṣata-hitā rakta-pittānilāpahāḥ ।
matsyaṇḍikā-khaṇḍa-sitāḥ krameṇa guṇa-vat-tamāḥ ।।

tad-guṇā tikta-madhurā kaṣāyā yāsa-śarkarā ।
dāha-tṛṭ-chardi-mūrchāsṛk-pitta-ghnyaḥ sarva-śarkarāḥ ।।

śarkarekṣu-vikārāṇāṃ phāṇitaṃ ca varāvare ।
cakṣuṣyaṃ chedi tṛṭ-śleṣma-viṣa-hidhmāsra-pitta-nut ।।

meha-kuṣṭha-kṛmi-cchardi-śvāsa-kāsātisāra-jit ।
vraṇa-śodhana-saṃdhāna-ropaṇaṃ vātalaṃ madhu ।।

rūkṣaṃ kaṣāya-madhuraṃ tat-tulyā madhu-śarkarā ।
uṣṇam uṣṇārtam uṣṇe ca yuktaṃ coṣṇair nihanti tat ।।
yakṣmārśo-'rdita-pittāsṛṅ-nāśanaṃ grāhi dīpanam ।।
pracchardane nirūhe ca madhūṣṇaṃ na nivāryate ।
a-labdha-pākam āśv eva tayor yasmān nivartate ।।

-labdha-pākam evāśu
tailaṃ sva-yoni-vat tatra mukhyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ vyavāyi ca ।
tvag-doṣa-kṛd a-cakṣuṣyaṃ sūkṣmoṣṇaṃ kapha-kṛn na ca ।।

kṛśānāṃ bṛṃhaṇāyālaṃ sthūlānāṃ karśanāya ca ।
baddha-viṭkaṃ kṛmi-ghnaṃ ca saṃskārāt sarva-roga-jit ।।

aṃskārāt sarva-doṣa-jit
sa-tiktoṣaṇam airaṇḍaṃ tailaṃ svādu saraṃ guru ।
vardhma-gulmānila-kaphān udaraṃ viṣama-jvaram ।।

ruk-śophau ca kaṭī-guhya-koṣṭha-pṛṣṭhāśrayau jayet ।
tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ picchilaṃ visraṃ raktairaṇḍodbhavaṃ tv ati ।।

kaṭūṣṇaṃ sārṣapaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ kapha-śukrānilāpaham ।
laghu pittāsra-kṛt koṭha-kuṣṭhārśo-vraṇa-jantu-jit ।।

ākṣaṃ svādu himaṃ keśyaṃ guru pittānilāpaham ।
nāty-uṣṇaṃ nimba-jaṃ tiktaṃ kṛmi-kuṣṭha-kapha-praṇut ।।

umā-kusumbha-jaṃ coṣṇaṃ tvag-doṣa-kapha-pitta-kṛt ।
vasā majjā ca vāta-ghnau bala-pitta-kapha-pradau ।।
kaṣāya-tikta-kaṭukaṃ kārañjaṃ vraṇa-śodhanam ।।
māṃsānuga-sva-rūpau ca vidyān medo api tāv iva ।
dīpanaṃ rocanaṃ madhyaṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ tuṣṭi-puṣṭi-dam ।।

sa-svādu-tikta-kaṭukam amla-pāka-rasaṃ saram ।
sa-kaṣāyaṃ svarārogya-pratibhā-varṇa-kṛl laghu ।।

naṣṭa-nidrāti-nidrebhyo hitaṃ pittāsra-dūṣaṇam ।
kṛśa-sthūla-hitaṃ rūkṣaṃ sūkṣmaṃ sroto-viśodhanam ।।

vāta-śleṣma-haraṃ yuktyā pītaṃ viṣa-vad anya-thā ।
guru tad-doṣa-jananaṃ navaṃ jīrṇam ato anya-thā ।।

drākṣekṣavaḥ sa-kharjūrāḥ śāli-piṣṭam yavasya ca ।
pañca madyākārāḥ śreṣṭhā drākṣā teṣāṃ viśiṣyate ।।

śāleḥ piṣṭam yavasya ca
peyaṃ noṣṇopacāreṇa na virikta-kṣudhāturaiḥ ।
nāty-artha-tīkṣṇa-mṛdv-alpa-saṃbhāraṃ kaluṣaṃ na ca ।।

gulmodarārśo-grahaṇī-śoṣa-hṛt snehanī guruḥ ।
surānila-ghnī medo-'sṛk-stanya-mūtra-kaphāvahā ।।

tad-guṇā vāruṇī hṛdyā laghus tīkṣṇā nihanti ca ।
śūla-kāsa-vami-śvāsa-vibandhādhmāna-pīnasān ।।

nāti-tīvra-madā laghvī pathyā vaibhītakī surā ।
vraṇe pāṇḍv-āmaye kuṣṭhe na cāty-arthaṃ virudhyate ।।

viṣṭambhinī yava-surā gurvī rūkṣā tri-doṣalā ।
yathā-dravya-guṇo ariṣṭaḥ sarva-madya-guṇādhikaḥ ।।

grahaṇī-pāṇḍu-kuṣṭhārśaḥ-śopha-śoṣodara-jvarān ।
hanti gulma-kṛmi-plīhnaḥ kaṣāya-kaṭu-vātalaḥ ।।

aṣāyaḥ kaṭu-vātalaḥ
mārdvīkaṃ lekhanaṃ hṛdyaṃ nāty-uṣṇaṃ madhuraṃ saram ।
alpa-pittānilaṃ pāṇḍu-mehārśaḥ-kṛmi-nāśanam ।।

asmād alpāntara-guṇaṃ khārjūraṃ vātalaṃ guru ।
śārkaraḥ surabhiḥ svādu-hṛdyo nāti-mado laghuḥ ।।

śārkaraṃ surabhi svādu ṛdyaṃ nāti-madaṃ laghu
sṛṣṭa-mūtra-śakṛd-vāto gauḍas tarpaṇa-dīpanaḥ ।
vāta-pitta-karaḥ sīdhuḥ sneha-śleṣma-vikāra-hā ।।

medaḥ-śophodarārśo-ghnas tatra pakva-raso varaḥ ।
chedī madhv-āsavas tīkṣṇo meha-pīnasa-kāsa-jit ।।

rakta-pitta-kaphotkledi śuktaṃ vātānulomanam ।
bhṛśoṣṇa-tīkṣṇa-rūkṣāmlaṃ hṛdyaṃ ruci-karaṃ saram ।।

ṛdyaṃ ruci-karaṃ param
dīpanaṃ śiśira-sparśaṃ pāṇḍu-dṛk-kṛmi-nāśanam ।
guḍekṣu-madya-mārdvīka-śuktaṃ laghu yathottaram ।।

āṇḍu-hṛt kṛmi-nāśanam uḍekṣu-madya-mādhvīka-
kanda-mūla-phalādyaṃ ca tad-vad vidyāt tad-āsutam ।
śāṇḍākī cāsutaṃ cānyat kālāmlaṃ rocanaṃ laghu ।।

dhānyāmlaṃ bhedi tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ pitta-kṛt sparśa-śītalam ।
śrama-klama-haraṃ rucyaṃ dīpanaṃ vasti-śūla-nut ।।

śastam āsthāpane hṛdyaṃ laghu vāta-kaphāpaham ।
ebhir eva guṇair yukte sauvīraka-tuṣodake ।।
gaṇḍūṣa-dhāraṇād vaktra-mala-daurgandhya-śoṣa-jit ।।
kṛmi-hṛd-roga-gulmārśaḥ-pāṇḍu-roga-nibarhaṇe ।
te kramād vi-tuṣair vidyāt sa-tuṣaiś ca yavaiḥ kṛte ।।

ṛmi-hṛd-roga-gulmārśo- -grahaṇī-pāṇḍu-nāśane
mūtraṃ go-'jāvi-mahiṣī-gajāśvoṣṭra-kharodbhavam ।
pittalaṃ rūkṣa-tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ lavaṇānu-rasaṃ kaṭu ।।

kṛmi-śophodarānāha-śūla-pāṇḍu-kaphānilān ।
gulmā-ruci-viṣa-śvitra-kuṣṭhārśāṃsi jayel laghu ।।

-śūla-pāṇḍu-kaphāmayān
toya-kṣīrekṣu-tailānāṃ vargair madyasya ca kramāt ।
iti dravaika-deśo ayaṃ yathā-sthūlam udāhṛtaḥ ।।

sūtrasthāna
rakto mahān sa-kalamas tūrṇakaḥ śakunāhṛtaḥ ।
sārā-mukho dīrghaśūko lodhraśūkaḥ sugandhikaḥ ।।

puṇḍraḥ pāṇḍuḥ puṇḍarīkaḥ pramodo gaura-śārivau ।
kāñcano mahiṣaḥ śūkaḥ dūṣakaḥ kusumāṇḍakaḥ ।।

āṇḍukaḥ puṇḍarīkaś ca auṇḍrakaḥ puṇḍarīkaś ca 
pramodo gaura-śālikaḥ
lāṅgalā lohavālākhyāḥ kardamāḥ śītabhīrukāḥ ।
pataṅgās tapanīyāś ca ye cānye śālayaḥ śubhāḥ ।।

āṅgalā lohavālākhyāḥ āṅgalā lohavālāś ca āṅgalo lohavālākhyaḥ 
ardamaḥ śītabhīrukaḥ
svādu-pāka-rasāḥ snigdhā vṛṣyā baddhālpa-varcasaḥ ।
kaṣāyānu-rasāḥ pathyā laghavo mūtralā himāḥ ।।

śūka-jeṣu varas tatra raktas tṛṣṇā-tri-doṣa-hā ।
mahāṃs tam anu kalamas taṃ cāpy anu tataḥ pare ।।

ahāṃs tasyānu kalamas
yavakā hāyanāḥ pāṃsu-bāṣpa-naiṣadhakādayaḥ ।
svādūṣṇā guravaḥ snigdhāḥ pāke amlāḥ śleṣma-pittalāḥ ।।

-vāpya-naiṣadhakādayaḥ
sṛṣṭa-mūtra-purīṣāś ca pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ ca ninditāḥ ।
snigdho grāhī laghuḥ svādus tri-doṣa-ghnaḥ sthiro himaḥ ।।

ṣaṣṭiko vrīhiṣu śreṣṭho gauraś cāsita-gaurataḥ ।
tataḥ kramān mahā-vrīhi-kṛṣṇa-vrīhi-jatūmukhāḥ ।।

kukkuṭāṇḍaka-lāvākhya-pārāvataka-śūkarāḥ ।
varakoddālakojjvāla-cīna-śārada-dardurāḥ ।।

ukkuṭāṇḍaka-pālākṣa- ukkuṭāṇḍaka-pālākhya- ukkuṭāṇḍaka-lāvākṣa- 
-cīna-śārada-durdarāḥ
gandhanāḥ kuruvindāś ca guṇair alpāntarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
svādur amla-vipāko anyo vrīhiḥ pitta-karo guruḥ ।।

bahu-mūtra-purīṣoṣmā tri-doṣas tv eva pāṭalaḥ ।
kaṅgu-kodrava-nīvāra-śyāmākādi himaṃ laghu ।।

tṛṇa-dhānyaṃ pavana-kṛl lekhanaṃ kapha-pitta-hṛt ।
bhagna-saṃdhāna-kṛt tatra priyaṅgur bṛṃhaṇī guruḥ ।।

koradūṣaḥ paraṃ grāhī sparśo śīto viṣāpahaḥ ।
rūkṣaḥ śīto guruḥ svāduḥ saro viḍ-vāta-kṛd yavaḥ ।।

parśo śīto garāpahaḥ parśa-śīto viṣāpahaḥ
vṛṣyaḥ sthairya-karo mūtra-medaḥ-pitta-kaphāñ jayet ।
pīnasa-śvāsa-kāsoru-stambha-kaṇṭha-tvag-āmayān ।।

nyūno yavād anu-yavo rūkṣoṣṇo vaṃśa-jo yavaḥ ।
vṛṣyaḥ śīto guruḥ snigdho jīvano vāta-pitta-hā ।।

yūno yāvad anya-yavo
saṃdhāna-kārī madhuro godhūmaḥ sthairya-kṛt saraḥ ।
pathyā nandīmukhī śītā kaṣāya-madhurā laghuḥ ।।
niḥ-sārā vātalā rūkṣā jūrṇādhmāna-karā sarā ।।
mudgāḍhakī-masūrādi śimbī-dhānyaṃ vibandha-kṛt ।
kaṣāyaṃ svādu saṃgrāhi kaṭu-pākaṃ himaṃ laghu ।।

medaḥ-śleṣmāsra-pitteṣu hitaṃ lepopasekayoḥ ।
varo atra mudgo alpa-calaḥ kalāyas tv ati-vātalaḥ ।।
asṛk-pitta-haro rūkṣo vātalaś caṇakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
rāja-māṣo anila-karo rūkṣo bahu-śakṛd guruḥ ।
uṣṇāḥ kulatthāḥ pāke amlāḥ śukrāśma-śvāsa-pīnasān ।।

kāsārśaḥ-kapha-vātāṃś ca ghnanti pittāsra-dāḥ param ।
niṣpāvo vāta-pittāsra-stanya-mūtra-karo guruḥ ।।

iṣpāvo vāta-pittāsṛk-
saro vidāhī dṛk-śukra-kapha-śopha-viṣāpahaḥ ।
māṣaḥ snigdho bala-śleṣma-mala-pitta-karaḥ saraḥ ।।

gurūṣṇo anila-hā svāduḥ śukra-vṛddhi-vireka-kṛt ।
phalāni māṣa-vad vidyāt kākāṇḍolātmaguptayoḥ ।।

uṣṇas tvacyo himaḥ sparśe keśyo balyas tilo guruḥ ।
alpa-mūtraḥ kaṭuḥ pāke medhāgni-kapha-pitta-kṛt ।।

ṣṇas tvacyo hima-sparśaḥ
snigdhomā svādu-tiktoṣṇā kapha-pitta-karī guruḥ ।
dṛk-śukra-hṛt kaṭuḥ pāke tad-vad bījaṃ kusumbha-jam ।।

māṣo atra sarveṣv avaro yavakaḥ śūka-jeṣu ca ।
navaṃ dhānyam abhiṣyandi laghu saṃvatsaroṣitam ।।

avakaḥ śūka-jeṣv api aghu varṣoṣitaṃ ca yat
śīghra-janma tathā sūpyaṃ nis-tuṣaṃ yukti-bharjitam ।
maṇḍa-peyā-vilepīnām odanasya ca lāghavam ।।

yava-godhūma-māṣāś ca tilāś cābhinavā hitāḥ ।
purāṇā vi-rasāḥ sūkṣmā na tathārtha-karā matāḥ ।।

yathā-pūrvaṃ śivas tatra maṇḍo vātānulomanaḥ ।
tṛḍ-glāni-doṣa-śeṣa-ghnaḥ pācano dhātu-sāmya-kṛt ।।

sroto-mārdava-kṛt svedī saṃdhukṣayati cānalam ।
kṣut-tṛṣṇā-glāni-daurbalya-kukṣi-roga-jvarāpahā ।।

malānulomanī pathyā peyā dīpana-pācanī ।
vilepī grāhiṇī hṛdyā tṛṣṇā-ghnī dīpanī hitā ।।

vraṇākṣi-roga-saṃśuddha-dur-bala-sneha-pāyinām ।
su-dhautaḥ prasrutaḥ svinno a-tyaktoṣmā caudano laghuḥ ।।

yaś cāgneyauṣadha-kvātha-sādhito bhṛṣṭa-taṇḍulaḥ ।
viparīto guruḥ kṣīra-māṃsādyair yaś ca sādhitaḥ ।।

aś cāgneyauṣadha-kvāthe ādhito bhṛṣṭa-taṇḍulaiḥ
iti dravya-kriyā-yoga-mānādyaiḥ sarvam ādiśet ।
bṛṃhaṇaḥ prīṇano vṛṣyaś cakṣuṣyo vraṇa-hā rasaḥ ।।

maudgas tu pathyaḥ saṃśuddha-vraṇa-kaṇṭhākṣi-rogiṇām ।
vātānulomī kaulattho gulma-tūṇī-pratūṇi-jit ।।

a-kṛtaṃ kṛta-yūṣaṃ ca tanu saṃskāritaṃ rasam ।
sūpam amlam an-amlaṃ ca guru vidyād yathottaram ।।

tila-piṇyāka-vikṛtiḥ śuṣka-śākaṃ virūḍhakam ।
śāṇḍākī-vaṭakaṃ dṛṅ-ghnaṃ doṣalaṃ glapanaṃ guru ।।

rasālā bṛṃhaṇī vṛṣyā snigdhā balyā ruci-pradā ।
śrama-kṣut-tṛṭ-klama-haraṃ pānakaṃ prīṇanaṃ guru ।।

viṣṭambhi mūtralaṃ hṛdyaṃ yathā-dravya-guṇaṃ ca tat ।
lājās tṛṭ-chardy-atīsāra-meha-medaḥ-kapha-cchidaḥ ।।

kāsa-pittopaśamanā dīpanā laghavo himāḥ ।
pṛthukā guravo balyāḥ kapha-viṣṭambha-kāriṇaḥ ।।

dhānā viṣṭambhinī rūkṣā tarpaṇī lekhanī guruḥ ।
saktavo laghavaḥ kṣut-tṛṭ-śrama-netrāmaya-vraṇān ।।

-śrama-netra-galāmayān
ghnanti saṃtarpaṇāḥ pānāt sadya eva bala-pradāḥ ।
nodakāntaritān na dvir na niśāyāṃ na kevalān ।।

na bhuktvā na dvi-jaiś chittvā saktūn adyān na vā bahūn ।
piṇyāko glapano rūkṣo viṣṭambhī dṛṣṭi-dūṣaṇaḥ ।।

raukṣyād viṣṭambhate koṣṭhe viṣṭambhi-tvād vidahyate ।
vidāhāt kurute glāniṃ piṇyāko niśi sevitaḥ ।।

vesavāro guruḥ snigdho balopacaya-vardhanaḥ ।
mudgādi-jās tu guravo yathā-dravya-guṇānugāḥ ।।

kukūla-karpara-bhrāṣṭra-kandv-aṅgāra-vipācitān ।
eka-yonīō̃ laghūn vidyād apūpān uttarottaram ।।

ukūla-kharpara-bhrāṣṭra- -kaṭv-aṅgāra-vipācitān 
apūpāṃs tu yathottaram
hariṇaiṇa-kuraṅgarkṣa-gokarṇa-mṛgamātṛkāḥ ।
śaśa-śambara-cāruṣka-śarabhādyā mṛgāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

lāva-vārtīka-vartīra-raktavartmaka-kukkubhāḥ ।
kapiñjalopacakrākhya-cakora-kurubāhavaḥ ।।

-raktavartmaka-kurkubhāḥ
vartako vartikā caiva tittiriḥ krakaraḥ śikhī ।
tāmra-cūḍākhya-bakara-gonarda-giri-vartikāḥ ।।

ukkuṭo bakaraḥ kaṅka- āmra-cūḍākhya-varaka-
tathā śārapadendrābha-varaṭādyāś ca viṣkirāḥ ।
jīvañjīvaka-dātyūha-bhṛṅgāhva-śuka-sārikāḥ ।।

-vāraṭādyāś ca viṣkirāḥ -vāraṭāś ceti viṣkirāḥ -varaṭāś 
ceti viṣkirāḥ
laṭvā-kokila-hārīta-kapota-caṭakādayaḥ ।
pratudā bheka-godhāhi-śvāvid-ādyā bile-śayāḥ ।।

go-kharāśvataroṣṭrāśva-dvīpi-siṃharkṣa-vānarāḥ ।
mārjāra-mūṣaka-vyāghra-vṛka-babhru-tarakṣavaḥ ।।

lopāka-jambuka-śyena-cāṣa-vāntāda-vāyasāḥ ।
śaśaghnī-bhāsa-kurara-gṛdhrolūka-kuliṅgakāḥ ।।

śaśāri-bhāsa-kurara-
dhūmikā madhuhā ceti prasahā mṛga-pakṣiṇaḥ ।
varāha-mahiṣa-nyaṅku-ruru-rohita-vāraṇāḥ ।।

sṛmaraś camaraḥ khaḍgo gavayaś ca mahā-mṛgāḥ ।
haṃsa-sārasa-kādamba-baka-kāraṇḍava-plavāḥ ।।

balākotkrośa-cakrāhva-madgu-krauñcādayo ap-carāḥ ।
matsyā rohita-pāṭhīna-kūrma-kumbhīra-karkaṭāḥ ।।

śukti-śaṅkhodra-śambūka-śapharī-varmi-candrikāḥ ।
culūkī-nakra-makara-śiśumāra-timiṅgilāḥ ।।

śukti-śaṅkhodru-śambūka- ullakī-nakra-makara-
rājī-cilicimādyāś ca māṃsam ity āhur aṣṭa-dhā ।
yoniṣv ajāvī vyāmiśra-go-cara-tvād a-niścite ।।

mṛgyaṃ vaiṣkirikaṃ kiṃ ca prātudaṃ ca bile-śayam ।
prāsahaṃ ca mahā-mṛgyam ap-caraṃ mātsyam aṣṭa-dhā ।।

ādyāntyā jāṅgalānūpā madhyau sādhāraṇau smṛtau ।
tatra baddha-malāḥ śītā laghavo jāṅgalā hitāḥ ।।

pittottare vāta-madhye saṃnipāte kaphānuge ।
dīpanaḥ kaṭukaḥ pāke grāhī rūkṣo himaḥ śaśaḥ ।।

īṣad-uṣṇa-guru-snigdhā bṛṃhaṇā vartakādayaḥ ।
tittiris teṣv api varo medhāgni-bala-śukra-kṛt ।।

grāhī varṇyo anilodrikta-saṃnipāta-haraḥ param ।
nāti-pathyaḥ śikhī pathyaḥ śrotra-svara-vayo-dṛśām ।।

tad-vac ca kukkuṭo vṛṣyo grāmyas tu śleṣmalo guruḥ ।
medhānala-karā hṛdyāḥ krakarāḥ sopacakrakāḥ ।।

guruḥ sa-lavaṇaḥ kāṇa-kapotaḥ sarva-doṣa-kṛt ।
caṭakāḥ śleṣmalāḥ snigdhā vāta-ghnāḥ śukralāḥ param ।।

āta-ghnāḥ śukralāḥ bhṛśam
gurūṣṇa-snigdha-madhurā vargāś cāto yathottaram ।
mūtra-śukra-kṛto balyā vāta-ghnāḥ kapha-pittalāḥ ।।

śītā mahā-mṛgās teṣu kravyāda-prasahāḥ punaḥ ।
lavaṇānu-rasāḥ pāke kaṭukā māṃsa-vardhanāḥ ।।

ravyādāḥ prasahāḥ punaḥ
jīrṇārśo-grahaṇī-doṣa-śoṣārtānāṃ paraṃ hitāḥ ।
nāti-śīta-guru-snigdhaṃ māṃsam ājam a-doṣalam ।।

āti-śītaṃ guru snigdhaṃ
śarīra-dhātu-sāmānyād an-abhiṣyandi bṛṃhaṇam ।
viparītam ato jñeyam āvikaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ tu tat ।।

śuṣka-kāsa-śramāty-agni-viṣama-jvara-pīnasān ।
kārśyaṃ kevala-vātāṃś ca go-māṃsaṃ saṃniyacchati ।।

uṣṇo garīyān mahiṣaḥ svapna-dārḍhya-bṛhat-tva-kṛt ।
tad-vad varāhaḥ śrama-hā ruci-śukra-bala-pradaḥ ।।

matsyāḥ paraṃ kapha-karāś cilicīmas tri-doṣa-kṛt ।
lāva-rohita-godhaiṇāḥ sve sve varge varāḥ param ।।

matsyādi-pakṣiṇāṃ caiva gurūṇy aṇḍāni cādiśet ।
tāni snigdhāni vṛṣyāṇi svādu-pāka-rasāni ca ।।

urūṇy aṇḍāny ato diśet urūṇy aṇḍāni cānyato
māṃsaṃ sadyo-hataṃ śuddhaṃ vayaḥ-sthaṃ ca bhajet tyajet ।
mṛtaṃ kṛśaṃ bhṛśaṃ medyaṃ vyādhi-vāri-viṣair hatam ।।

puṃ-striyoḥ pūrva-paścārdhe guruṇī garbhiṇī guruḥ ।
laghur yoṣic catuṣ-pātsu vihaṅgeṣu punaḥ pumān ।।

śiraḥ-skandhoru-pṛṣṭhasya kaṭyāḥ sakthnoś ca gauravam ।
tathāma-pakvāśayayor yathā-pūrvaṃ vinirdiśet ।।

śoṇita-prabhṛtīnāṃ ca dhātūnām uttarottaram ।
māṃsād garīyo vṛṣaṇa-meḍhra-vṛkka-yakṛd-gudam ।।

śākaṃ pāṭhā-śaṭhī-sūṣā-suniṣaṇṇa-satīna-jam ।
tri-doṣa-ghnaṃ laghu grāhi sa-rāja-kṣava-vāstukam ।।

śākaṃ pāṭhā-śaṭhī-śūṣā-
suniṣaṇṇo agni-kṛd vṛṣyas teṣu rāja-kṣavaḥ param ।
grahaṇy-arśo-vikāra-ghno varco-bhedi tu vāstukam ।।

hanti doṣa-trayaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ vṛṣyā soṣṇā rasāyanī ।
kākamācī sarā svaryā cāṅgery amlāgni-dīpanī ।।

ṛṣyā soṣṇā rasāyanam
grahaṇy-arśo-'nila-śleṣman-hitoṣṇā grāhiṇī laghuḥ ।
paṭola-saptalāriṣṭa-śārṅgaṣṭāvalgujāmṛtāḥ ।।

aṭolaṃ saptalāriṣṭa-
vetrāgra-bṛhatī-vāsā-kutilī-tilaparṇikāḥ ।
maṇḍūkaparṇī-karkoṭa-kāravellaka-parpaṭāḥ ।।

etrāgraṃ bṛhatī-vāsā- -kuntilī-tilaparṇikāḥ 
-kuntalī-tilaparṇikāḥ
nāḍī-kalāya-gojihvā-vārtākaṃ vanatiktakam ।
karīraṃ kulakaṃ nandī kucailā śakulādanī ।।

kaṭhillaṃ kembukaṃ śītaṃ sa-kośātaka-karkaśam ।
tiktaṃ pāke kaṭu grāhi vātalaṃ kapha-pitta-jit ।।

aṭhilla-kembukaṃ śītaṃ
hṛdyaṃ paṭolaṃ kṛmi-nut svādu-pākaṃ ruci-pradam ।
pittalaṃ dīpanaṃ bhedi vāta-ghnaṃ bṛhatī-dvayam ।।

vṛṣaṃ tu vami-kāsa-ghnaṃ rakta-pitta-haraṃ param ।
kāravellaṃ sa-kaṭukaṃ dīpanaṃ kapha-jit param ।।

vārtākaṃ kaṭu-tiktoṣṇaṃ madhuraṃ kapha-vāta-jit ।
sa-kṣāram agni-jananaṃ hṛdyaṃ rucyam a-pittalam ।।

karīram ādhmāna-karaṃ kaṣāyaṃ svādu tiktakam ।
kośātakāvalgujakau bhedināv agni-dīpanau ।।

hedanāv agni-dīpanau
taṇḍulīyo himo rūkṣaḥ svādu-pāka-raso laghuḥ ।
mada-pitta-viṣāsra-ghno muñjātaṃ vāta-pitta-jit ।।

snigdhaṃ śītaṃ guru svādu bṛṃhaṇaṃ śukra-kṛt param ।
gurvī sarā tu pālaṅkyā mada-ghnī cāpy upodakā ।।

pālaṅkyā-vat smṛtaś cañcuḥ sa tu saṃgrahaṇātmakaḥ ।
vidārī vāta-pitta-ghnī mūtralā svādu-śītalā ।।

ālaṅkyā-vat smṛtaś cuccuḥ ālaṅkyā-vat smṛtaś cuñcuḥ
jīvanī bṛṃhaṇī kaṇṭhyā gurvī vṛṣyā rasāyanam ।
cakṣuṣyā sarva-doṣa-ghnī jīvantī madhurā himā ।।

kūṣmāṇḍa-tumba-kāliṅga-karkārv-ervāru-tiṇḍiśam ।
tathā trapusa-cīnāka-cirbhaṭaṃ kapha-vāta-kṛt ।।

bhedi viṣṭambhy abhiṣyandi svādu-pāka-rasaṃ guru ।
vallī-phalānāṃ pravaraṃ kūṣmāṇḍaṃ vāta-pitta-jit ।।

vasti-śuddhi-karaṃ vṛṣyaṃ trapusaṃ tv ati-mūtralam ।
tumbaṃ rūkṣa-taraṃ grāhi kāliṅgairvāru-cirbhaṭam ।।

bālaṃ pitta-haraṃ śītaṃ vidyāt pakvam ato anya-thā ।
śīrṇavṛntaṃ tu sa-kṣāraṃ pittalaṃ kapha-vāta-jit ।।

rocanaṃ dīpanaṃ hṛdyam aṣṭhīlānāha-nul laghu ।
mṛṇāla-bisa-śālūka-kumudotpala-kandakam ।।

nandī-māṣaka-kelūṭa-śṛṅgāṭaka-kaserukam ।
krauñcādanaṃ kaloḍyaṃ ca rūkṣaṃ grāhi himaṃ guru ।।

kadamba-nālikā-mārṣa-kuṭiñjara-kutumbakam ।
cillī-laṭvāka-loṇīkā-kurūṭaka-gavedhukam ।।

alambu-nālikā-mārṣa- -kuṭiñjara-kurumbakam -kuliñjara-kurumbakam -kurūḍhaka-gavedhukāḥ -kuraṇṭaka-gavedhukāḥ 
-kuraṇṭaka-gavedhukam
jīvanta-jhuñjhv-eḍagaja-yava-śāka-suvarcalāḥ ।
ālukāni ca sarvāṇi tathā sūpyāni lakṣmaṇam ।।

-yava-śāka-suvarcalam athā sūpyāni lākṣmaṇam athā 
sūpyāni lakṣmaṇā
svādu rūkṣaṃ sa-lavaṇaṃ vāta-śleṣma-karaṃ guru ।
śītalaṃ sṛṣṭa-viṇ-mūtraṃ prāyo viṣṭabhya jīryati ।।

svinnaṃ niṣpīḍita-rasaṃ snehāḍhyaṃ nāti-doṣalam ।
laghu-pattrā tu yā cillī sā vāstuka-samā matā ।।

tarkārī-varuṇaṃ svādu sa-tiktaṃ kapha-vāta-jit ।
varṣābhvau kāla-śākaṃ ca sa-kṣāraṃ kaṭu-tiktakam ।।

arkārī-varaṇaṃ svādu
dīpanaṃ bhedanaṃ hanti gara-śopha-kaphānilān ।
dīpanāḥ kapha-vāta-ghnāś ciribilvāṅkurāḥ sarāḥ ।।
saṃgrāhi śālmalī-puṣpaṃ pittāsra-ghnaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
śatāvary-aṅkurās tiktā vṛṣyā doṣa-trayāpahāḥ ।
rūkṣo vaṃśa-karīras tu vidāhī vāta-pittalaḥ ।।

pattūro dīpanas tiktaḥ plīhārśaḥ-kapha-vāta-jit ।
kṛmi-kāsa-kaphotkledān kāsamardo jayet saraḥ ।।

rūkṣoṣṇam amlaṃ kausumbhaṃ guru pitta-karaṃ saram ।
gurūṣṇaṃ sārṣapaṃ baddha-viṇ-mūtraṃ sarva-doṣa-kṛt ।।

yad bālam a-vyakta-rasaṃ kiñ-cit-kṣāraṃ sa-tiktakam ।
tan mūlakaṃ doṣa-haraṃ laghu soṣṇaṃ niyacchati ।।

gulma-kāsa-kṣaya-śvāsa-vraṇa-netra-galāmayān ।
svarāgni-sādodāvarta-pīnasāṃś ca mahat punaḥ ।।

rase pāke ca kaṭukam uṣṇa-vīryaṃ tri-doṣa-kṛt ।
gurv abhiṣyandi ca snigdha-siddhaṃ tad api vāta-jit ।।

-svinnaṃ tad api vāta-jit
vāta-śleṣma-haraṃ śuṣkaṃ sarvam āmaṃ tu doṣalam ।
kaṭūṣṇo vāta-kapha-hā piṇḍāluḥ pitta-vardhanaḥ ।।

kuṭhera-śigru-surasa-sumukhāsuri-bhūstṛṇam ।
phaṇijjārjaka-jambīra-prabhṛti grāhi śālanam ।।

vidāhi kaṭu rūkṣoṣṇaṃ hṛdyaṃ dīpana-rocanam ।
dṛk-śukra-kṛmi-hṛt tīkṣṇaṃ doṣotkleśa-karaṃ laghu ।।

hidhmā-kāsa-viṣa-śvāsa-pārśva-ruk-pūti-gandha-hā ।
surasaḥ sumukho nāti-vidāhī gara-śopha-hā ।।

idhmā-kāsa-vami-śvāsa- idhmā-kāsa-śrama-śvāsa-
ārdrikā tikta-madhurā mūtralā na ca pitta-kṛt ।
laśuno bhṛśa-tīkṣṇoṣṇaḥ kaṭu-pāka-rasaḥ saraḥ ।।

hṛdyaḥ keśyo gurur vṛṣyaḥ snigdho rocana-dīpanaḥ ।
bhagna-saṃdhāna-kṛd balyo rakta-pitta-pradūṣaṇaḥ ।।

nigdho dīpana-pācanaḥ
kilāsa-kuṣṭha-gulmārśo-meha-kṛmi-kaphānilān ।
sa-hidhmā-pīnasa-śvāsa-kāsān hanti rasāyanam ।।

-kāsān hanty asra-pitta-kṛt
palāṇḍus tad-guṇa-nyūnaḥ śleṣmalo nāti-pittalaḥ ।
kapha-vātārśasāṃ pathyaḥ svede abhyavahṛtau tathā ।।

tīkṣṇo gṛñjanako grāhī pittināṃ hita-kṛn na saḥ ।
dīpanaḥ sūraṇo rucyaḥ kapha-ghno viśado laghuḥ ।।

viśeṣād arśasāṃ pathyo bhū-kandas tv ati-doṣalaḥ ।
pattre puṣpe phale nāle kande ca guru-tā kramāt ।।

uṣpe pattre phale nāle
varā śākeṣu jīvantī sārṣapaṃ tv avaraṃ param ।
drākṣā phalottamā vṛṣyā cakṣuṣyā sṛṣṭa-mūtra-viṭ ।।

ārṣapas tv avaraḥ param arṣapās tv avarāḥ param
svādu-pāka-rasā snigdhā sa-kaṣāyā himā guruḥ ।
nihanty anila-pittāsra-tiktāsya-tva-madātyayān ।।

ihanty anila-pittāsṛk-
tṛṣṇā-kāsa-śrama-śvāsa-svara-bheda-kṣata-kṣayān ।
udrikta-pittāñ jayati trīn doṣān svādu dāḍimam ।।

pittā-virodhi nāty-uṣṇam amlaṃ vāta-kaphāpaham ।
sarvaṃ hṛdyaṃ laghu snigdhaṃ grāhi rocana-dīpanam ।।

moca-kharjūra-panasa-nārikela-parūṣakam ।
āmrāta-tāla-kāśmarya-rājādana-madhūka-jam ।।

sauvīra-badarāṅkolla-phalgu-śleṣmātakodbhavam ।
vātāmābhiṣukākṣoṭa-mukūlaka-nikocakam ।।

urumāṇaṃ priyālaṃ ca bṛṃhaṇaṃ guru śītalam ।
dāha-kṣata-kṣaya-haraṃ rakta-pitta-prasādanam ।।

svādu-pāka-rasaṃ snigdhaṃ viṣṭambhi kapha-śukra-kṛt ।
phalaṃ tu pittalaṃ tālaṃ saraṃ kāśmarya-jaṃ himam ।।

śleṣmalaṃ vāta-pitta-jit
śakṛn-mūtra-vibandha-ghnaṃ keśyaṃ medhyaṃ rasāyanam ।
vātāmādy uṣṇa-vīryaṃ tu kapha-pitta-karaṃ saram ।।

paraṃ vāta-haraṃ snigdham an-uṣṇaṃ tu priyāla-jam ।
priyāla-majjā madhuro vṛṣyaḥ pittānilāpahaḥ ।।

kola-majjā guṇais tad-vat tṛṭ-chardiḥ-kāsa-jic ca saḥ ।
pakvaṃ su-dur-jaraṃ bilvaṃ doṣalaṃ pūti-mārutam ।।

dīpanaṃ kapha-vāta-ghnaṃ bālaṃ grāhy ubhayaṃ ca tat ।
kapittham āmaṃ kaṇṭha-ghnaṃ doṣalaṃ doṣa-ghāti tu ।।

ālaṃ grāhy ubhayaṃ tu tat
pakvaṃ hidhmā-vamathu-jit sarvaṃ grāhi viṣāpaham ।
jāmbavaṃ guru viṣṭambhi śītalaṃ bhṛśa-vātalam ।।

saṃgrāhi mūtra-śakṛtor a-kaṇṭhyaṃ kapha-pitta-jit ।
vāta-pittāsra-kṛd bālaṃ baddhāsthi kapha-pitta-kṛt ।।

-kaṇṭhyaṃ kapha-pitta-nut
gurv āmraṃ vāta-jit pakvaṃ svāamlaṃ kapha-śukra-kṛt ।
vṛkṣāmlaṃ grāhi rūkṣoṣṇaṃ vāta-śleṣma-haraṃ laghu ।।
tṛṣṇā-ghnam uṣṇam amlāyāḥ phalaṃ pitta-karaṃ saram ।।
śamyā gurūṣṇaṃ keśa-ghnaṃ rūkṣaṃ pīlu tu pittalam ।
kapha-vāta-haraṃ bhedi plīhārśaḥ-kṛmi-gulma-nut ।।

sa-tiktaṃ svādu yat pīlu nāty-uṣṇaṃ tat tri-doṣa-jit ।
tvak tikta-kaṭukā snigdhā mātuluṅgasya vāta-jit ।।

bṛṃhaṇaṃ madhuraṃ māṃsaṃ vāta-pitta-haraṃ guru ।
laghu tat-kesaraṃ kāsa-śvāsa-hidhmā-madātyayān ।।

āsya-śoṣānila-śleṣma-vibandha-cchardy-a-rocakān ।
gulmodarārśaḥ-śūlāni mandāgni-tvaṃ ca nāśayet ।।

madhuraṃ kiñ-cid amlaṃ ca hṛdyaṃ bhakta-prarocakam ।
guru vāta-praśamanaṃ vidyān nāraṅga-jaṃ phalam ।।

bhallātakasya tvaṅ-māṃsaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ svādu śītalam ।
tad-asthy-agni-samaṃ medhyaṃ kapha-vāta-haraṃ param ।।

svāamlaṃ śītam uṣṇaṃ ca dvi-dhā pālevataṃ guru ।
rucyam aty-agni-śamanaṃ rucyaṃ madhuram ārukam ।।

ṛdyaṃ madhuram ārukam
pakvam āśu jarāṃ yāti nāty-uṣṇa-guru-doṣalam ।
drākṣā-parūṣakaṃ cārdram amlaṃ pitta-kapha-pradam ।।

āty-uṣṇaṃ guru doṣalam
gurūṣṇa-vīryaṃ vāta-ghnaṃ saraṃ sa-karamardakam ।
tathāmlaṃ kola-karkandhu-likucāmrātakārukam ।।

ad-vac ca kola-karkandhu- -likucāmrātam ārukam
airāvataṃ dantaśaṭhaṃ sa-tūdaṃ mṛgaliṇḍikam ।
nāti-pitta-karaṃ pakvaṃ śuṣkaṃ ca karamardakam ।।

dīpanaṃ bhedanaṃ śuṣkam amlīkā-kolayoḥ phalam ।
tṛṣṇā-śrama-klama-cchedi laghv iṣṭaṃ kapha-vātayoḥ ।।
svāamlaṃ laghu kolaṃ tu śuṣkaṃ jīrṇaṃ ca dīpanam ।।
phalānām avaraṃ tatra likucaṃ sarva-doṣa-kṛt ।
himānaloṣṇa-dur-vāta-vyāla-lālādi-dūṣitam ।।

imāniloṣṇa-dur-vāta-
vāta-ghnaṃ dur-jaraṃ proktaṃ nāraṅgaṃ kapha-kṛd guru ।
tṛṣṇā-śūla-kaphotkleda-cchardi-śvāsa-nivāraṇam ।।

nārikelaṃ guru snigdhaṃ pitta-ghnaṃ svādu śītalam ।
bala-māṃsa-karaṃ hṛdyaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ vasti-śodhanam ।।

jantu-juṣṭaṃ jale magnam a-bhūmi-jam an-ārtavam ।
anya-dhānya-yutaṃ hīna-vīryaṃ jīrṇa-tayāti ca ।।

-vīryaṃ jīrṇa-tayāpi ca
dhānyaṃ tyajet tathā śākaṃ rūkṣa-siddham a-komalam ।
a-saṃjāta-rasaṃ tad-vac chuṣkaṃ cānya-tra mūlakāt ।।

prāyeṇa phalam apy evaṃ tathāmaṃ bilva-varjitam ।
viṣyandi lavaṇaṃ sarvaṃ sūkṣmaṃ sṛṣṭa-malaṃ viduḥ ।।

ūkṣmaṃ sṛṣṭa-malaṃ mṛdu
vāta-ghnaṃ pāki tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ rocanaṃ kapha-pitta-kṛt ।
saindhavaṃ tatra sa-svādu vṛṣyaṃ hṛdyaṃ tri-doṣa-nut ।।

laghv an-uṣṇaṃ dṛśaḥ pathyam a-vidāhy agni-dīpanam ।
laghu sauvarcalaṃ hṛdyaṃ su-gandhy udgāra-śodhanam ।।

kaṭu-pākaṃ vibandha-ghnaṃ dīpanīyaṃ ruci-pradam ।
ūrdhvādhaḥ-kapha-vātānulomanaṃ dīpanaṃ viḍam ।।

aṭu pāke vibandha-ghnaṃ
vibandhānāha-viṣṭambha-śūla-gaurava-nāśanam ।
vipāke svādu sāmudraṃ guru śleṣma-vivardhanam ।।

sa-tikta-kaṭuka-kṣāraṃ tīkṣṇam utkledi caudbhidam ।
kṛṣṇe sauvarcala-guṇā lavaṇe gandha-varjitāḥ ।।

romakaṃ laghu pāṃsūtthaṃ sa-kṣāraṃ śleṣmalaṃ guru ।
lavaṇānāṃ prayoge tu saindhavādi prayojayet ।।

aindhavādīn prayojayet
gulma-hṛd-grahaṇī-pāṇḍu-plīhānāha-galāmayān ।
śvāsārśaḥ-kapha-kāsāṃś ca śamayed yava-śūka-jaḥ ।।

śvāsārśaḥ-kapha-vātāṃś ca śamayed yāva-śūka-jaḥ
kṣāraḥ sarvaś ca paramaṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇaḥ kṛmi-jil laghuḥ ।
pittāsṛg-dūṣaṇaḥ pākī chedy a-hṛdyo vidāraṇaḥ ।।

a-pathyaḥ kaṭu-lāvaṇyāc chukraujaḥ-keśa-cakṣuṣām ।
hiṅgu vāta-kaphānāha-śūla-ghnaṃ pitta-kopanam ।।

kaṭu-pāka-rasaṃ rucyaṃ dīpanaṃ pācanaṃ laghu ।
kaṣāyā madhurā pāke rūkṣā vi-lavaṇā laghuḥ ।।

dīpanī pācanī medhyā vayasaḥ sthāpanī param ।
uṣṇa-vīryā sarāyuṣyā buddhīndriya-bala-pradā ।।

kuṣṭha-vaivarṇya-vaisvarya-purāṇa-viṣama-jvarān ।
śiro-'kṣi-pāṇḍu-hṛd-roga-kāmalā-grahaṇī-gadān ।।

sa-śoṣa-śophātīsāra-meda-moha-vami-kṛmīn ।
śvāsa-kāsa-prasekārśaḥ-plīhānāha-garodaram ।।

-meha-moha-vami-kṛmīn
vibandhaṃ srotasāṃ gulmam ūru-stambham a-rocakam ।
harītakī jayed vyādhīṃs tāṃs tāṃś ca kapha-vāta-jān ।।

tad-vad āmalakaṃ śītam amlaṃ pitta-kaphāpaham ।
kaṭu pāke himaṃ keśyam akṣam īṣac ca tad-guṇam ।।

aṭu pāke a-himaṃ keśyam
iyaṃ rasāyana-varā tri-phalākṣy-āmayāpahā ।
ropaṇī tvag gada-kleda-medo-meha-kaphāsra-jit ।।

sa-kesaraṃ catur-jātaṃ tvak-pattrailaṃ tri-jātakam ।
pitta-prakopi tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ rocana-dīpanam ।।

su-gandhi sarva-peyānāṃ vyañjanānāṃ ca vāsanam ।
lehānāṃ khādya-pākānāṃ cūrṇānāṃ ca prayojayet ।।

rase pāke ca kaṭukaṃ kapha-ghnaṃ maricaṃ laghu ।
śleṣmalā svādu-śītārdrā gurvī snigdhā ca pippalī ।।

sā śuṣkā viparītātaḥ snigdhā vṛṣyā rase kaṭuḥ ।
svādu-pākānila-śleṣma-śvāsa-kāsāpahā sarā ।।

na tām aty upayuñjīta rasāyana-vidhiṃ vinā ।
nāgaraṃ dīpanaṃ vṛṣyaṃ grāhi hṛdyaṃ vibandha-nut ।।

rucyaṃ laghu svādu-pākaṃ snigdhoṣṇaṃ kapha-vāta-jit ।
tad-vad ārdrakam etac ca trayaṃ tri-kaṭukaṃ jayet ।।

sthaulyāgni-sadana-śvāsa-kāsa-ślīpada-pīnasān ।
cavikā-pippalī-mūlaṃ maricālpāntaraṃ guṇaiḥ ।।

citrako agni-samaḥ pāke śophārśaḥ-kṛmi-kuṣṭha-hā ।
pañca-kolakam etac ca maricena vinā smṛtam ।।

añca-kolakam etat tu
gulma-plīhodarānāha-śūla-ghnaṃ dīpanaṃ param ।
bilva-kāśmarya-tarkārī-pāṭalā-ṭuṇṭukair mahat ।।

-śūla-ghnaṃ dīpanaṃ laghu
jayet kaṣāya-tiktoṣṇaṃ pañca-mūlaṃ kaphānilau ।
hrasvaṃ bṛhaty-aṃśumatī-dvaya-gokṣurakaiḥ smṛtam ।।

ayet kaṣāya-tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ
svādu-pāka-rasaṃ nāti-śītoṣṇaṃ sarva-doṣa-jit ।
balā-punarnavairaṇḍa-śūrpaparṇī-dvayena tu ।।

alā-punarnavairaṇḍaiḥ -śūrpaparṇī-dvayena ca śūrpaparṇī-dvayena ca 
śūrpaparṇī-dvayena tu
madhyamaṃ kapha-vāta-ghnaṃ nāti-pitta-karaṃ saram ।
abhīru-vīrā-jīvantī-jīvakarṣabhakaiḥ smṛtam ।।

jīvanākhyaṃ tu cakṣuṣyaṃ vṛṣyaṃ pittānilāpaham ।
tṛṇākhyaṃ pitta-jid darbha-kāśekṣu-śara-śālibhiḥ ।।

īvanākhyaṃ ca cakṣuṣyaṃ
śūka-śimbī-ja-pakvānna-māṃsa-śāka-phalauṣadhaiḥ ।
vargitair anna-leśo ayam ukto nityopayogikaḥ ।।

kto nityaupayogikaḥ

sūtrasthāna
rājā rāja-gṛhāsanne prāṇācāryaṃ niveśayet ।
sarva-dā sa bhavaty evaṃ sarva-tra pratijāgṛviḥ ।।

anna-pānaṃ viṣād rakṣed viśeṣeṇa mahī-pateḥ ।
yoga-kṣemau tad-āyattau dharmādyā yan-nibandhanāḥ ।।

harmādyās tan-nibandhanāḥ
odano viṣa-vān sāndro yāty a-visrāvya-tām iva ।
cireṇa pacyate pakvo bhavet paryuṣitopamaḥ ।।

mayūra-kaṇṭha-tulyoṣmā moha-mūrchā-praseka-kṛt ।
hīyate varṇa-gandhādyaiḥ klidyate candrikā-citaḥ ।।

lidyate candrikānvitaḥ lidyate candrakācitaḥ 
lidyate candrakānvitaḥ
vyañjanāny āśu śuṣyanti dhyāma-kvāthāni tatra ca ।
hīnātiriktā vikṛtā chāyā dṛśyeta naiva vā ।।

hāyā dṛśyeta vā na vā
phenordhva-rāji-sīmanta-tantu-budbuda-saṃbhavaḥ ।
vicchinna-vi-rasāḥ rāgāḥ khāṇḍavāḥ śākam āmiṣam ।।

icchinna-vi-rasā rāga- icchinnā vi-rasā rāgāḥ -khāṇḍavāḥ 
śākam āmiṣam
nīlā rājī rase tāmrā kṣīre dadhani dṛśyate ।
śyāvā-pītāsitā takre ghṛte pānīya-saṃnibhā ।।

ṣīre dadhni ca dṛśyate
mastuni syāt kapotābhā rājī kṛṣṇā tuṣodake ।
kālī madyāmbhasoḥ kṣaudre harit taile aruṇopamā ।।

pākaḥ phalānām āmānāṃ pakvānāṃ parikothanam ।
dravyāṇām ārdra-śuṣkāṇāṃ syātāṃ mlāni-vivarṇa-te ।।

mṛdūnāṃ kaṭhinānāṃ ca bhavet sparśa-viparyayaḥ ।
mālyasya sphuṭitāgra-tvaṃ mlānir gandhāntarodbhavaḥ ।।

ālyānāṃ sphuṭitāgra-tvaṃ lānir gandhāntarodbhavaḥ 
mlāni-gandhāntarodbhavaḥ
dhyāma-maṇḍala-tā vastre śadanaṃ tantu-pakṣmaṇām ।
dhātu-mauktika-kāṣṭhāśma-ratnādiṣu malākta-tā ।।

śātanaṃ tantu-pakṣmaṇām
sneha-sparśa-prabhā-hāniḥ sa-prabha-tvaṃ tu mṛn-maye ।
viṣa-daḥ śyāva-śuṣkāsyo vi-lakṣo vīkṣate diśaḥ ।।

sveda-vepathu-māṃs trasto bhītaḥ skhalati jṛmbhate ।
prāpyānnaṃ sa-viṣaṃ tv agnir ekāvartaḥ sphuṭaty ati ।।

kāvartaḥ sphuṭaty api
śikhi-kaṇṭhābha-dhūmārcir an-arcir vogra-gandha-vān ।
mriyante makṣikāḥ prāśya kākaḥ kṣāma-svaro bhavet ।।

utkrośanti ca dṛṣṭvaitac chuka-dātyūha-sārikāḥ ।
haṃsaḥ praskhalati glānir jīvañjīvasya jāyate ।।

cakorasyākṣi-vairāgyaṃ krauñcasya syān madodayaḥ ।
kapota-parabhṛd-dakṣa-cakravākā jahaty asūn ।।

udvegaṃ yāti mārjāraḥ śakṛn muñcati vānaraḥ ।
hṛṣyen mayūras tad-dṛṣṭyā manda-tejo bhaved viṣam ।।

dvejayati mārjāraḥ ṛṣyen mayūras tad dṛṣṭvā
ity annaṃ viṣa-vaj jñātvā tyajed evaṃ prayatnataḥ ।
yathā tena vipadyerann api na kṣudra-jantavaḥ ।।

ty annaṃ sa-viṣaṃ jñātvā yajed eva prayatnataḥ
spṛṣṭe tu kaṇḍū-dāhoṣā-jvarārti-sphoṭa-suptayaḥ ।
nakha-roma-cyutiḥ śophaḥ sekādyā viṣa-nāśanāḥ ।।

śastās tatra pralepāś ca sevya-candana-padmakaiḥ ।
sa-somavalka-tālīśa-pattra-kuṣṭhāmṛtā-nataiḥ ।।

lālā jihvauṣṭhayor jāḍyam ūṣā cimicimāyanam ।
danta-harṣo rasā-jña-tvaṃ hanu-stambhaś ca vaktra-ge ।।

ālā jihvauṣṭhayor jāḍyaṃ ukhe cimicimāyanam
sevyādyais tatra gaṇḍūṣāḥ sarvaṃ ca viṣa-jid dhitam ।
āmāśaya-gate sveda-mūrchādhmāna-mada-bhramāḥ ।।

roma-harṣo vamir dāhaś cakṣur-hṛdaya-rodhanam ।
bindubhiś cācayo aṅgānāṃ pakvāśaya-gate punaḥ ।।

aneka-varṇaṃ vamati mūtrayaty atisāryate ।
tandrā kṛśa-tvaṃ pāṇḍu-tvam udaraṃ bala-saṃkṣayaḥ ।।

tayor vānta-viriktasya haridre kaṭabhīṃ guḍam ।
sindhuvārita-niṣpāva-bāṣpikā-śataparvikāḥ ।।

taṇḍulīyaka-mūlāni kukkuṭāṇḍam avalgujam ।
nāvanāñjana-pāneṣu yojayed viṣa-śāntaye ।।

viṣa-bhuktāya dadyāc ca śuddhāyordhvam adhas tathā ।
sūkṣmaṃ tāmra-rajaḥ kāle sa-kṣaudraṃ hṛd-viśodhanam ।।

śuddhe hṛdi tataḥ śāṇaṃ hema-cūrṇasya dāpayet ।
na sajjate hema-pāṅge padma-pattre ambu-vad viṣam ।।

jāyate vipulaṃ cāyur gare apy eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।
viruddham api cāhāraṃ vidyād viṣa-garopamam ।।

idyād gara-viṣopamam
ānūpam āmiṣaṃ māṣa-kṣaudra-kṣīra-virūḍhakaiḥ ।
virudhyate saha bisair mūlakena guḍena vā ।।

viśeṣāt payasā matsyā matsyeṣv api cilīcimaḥ ।
viruddham amlaṃ payasā saha sarvaṃ phalaṃ tathā ।।

tad-vat kulattha-caṇaka-kaṅgu-valla-makuṣṭakāḥ ।
bhakṣayitvā haritakaṃ mūlakādi payas tyajet ।।

ad-vat kulattha-varaka- hakṣayitvā harit-kanda- 
-mūlakādi payas tyajet
vārāhaṃ śvāvidhā nādyād dadhnā pṛṣata-kukkuṭau ।
āma-māṃsāni pittena māṣa-sūpena mūlakam ।।

arāhaṃ śvāvidhā nādyād
aviṃ kusumbha-śākena bisaiḥ saha virūḍhakam ।
māṣa-sūpa-guḍa-kṣīra-dadhy-ājyair lākucaṃ phalam ।।

phalaṃ kadalyās takreṇa dadhnā tāla-phalena vā ।
kaṇoṣaṇābhyāṃ madhunā kākamācīṃ guḍena vā ।।

siddhāṃ vā matsya-pacane pacane nāgarasya vā ।
siddhām anya-tra vā pātre kāmāt tām uṣitāṃ niśām ।।

acane nāgarasya ca āmāt tām uṣitāṃ niśi apotām uṣitāṃ niśām ādyāt tām uṣitāṃ niśām āmātām uṣitāṃ niśām 
kāmācīm uṣitāṃ niśām
matsya-nistalana-snehe sādhitāḥ pippalīs tyajet ।
kāṃsye daśāham uṣitaṃ sarpir uṣṇaṃ tv aruṣkare ।।

atsya-nistalana-sneha- -sādhitāḥ pippalīs tyajet arpir 
uṣṇaṃ tv aruṣkaraiḥ
bhāso virudhyate śūlyaḥ kampillas takra-sādhitaḥ ।
aikadhyaṃ pāyasa-surā-kṛśarāḥ parivarjayet ।।

madhu-sarpir-vasā-taila-pānīyāni dvi-śaś tri-śaḥ ।
eka-tra vā samāṃśāni virudhyante paras-param ।।

bhinnāṃśe api madhv-ājye divya-vāry anu-pānataḥ ।
madhu-puṣkara-bījaṃ ca madhu-maireya-śārkaram ।।

manthānu-pānaḥ kṣaireyo hāridraḥ kaṭu-taila-vān ।
upodakātisārāya tila-kalkena sādhitā ।।

balākā vāruṇī-yuktā kulmāṣaiś ca virudhyate ।
bhṛṣṭā varāha-vasayā saiva sadyo nihanty asūn ।।

tad-vat tittiri-pattrāḍhya-godhā-lāva-kapiñjalāḥ ।
airaṇḍenāgninā siddhās tat-tailena vimūrchitāḥ ।।

hārīta-māṃsaṃ hāridra-śūlaka-prota-pācitam ।
haridrā-vahninā sadyo vyāpādayati jīvitam ।।

āridra-vahninā sadyo
bhasma-pāṃsu-paridhvastaṃ tad eva ca sa-mākṣikam ।
yat kiñ-cid doṣam utkleśya na haret tat samāsataḥ ।।

viruddhaṃ śuddhir atreṣṭā śamo vā tad-virodhibhiḥ ।
dravyais tair eva vā pūrvaṃ śarīrasyābhisaṃskṛtiḥ ।।

vyāyāma-snigdha-dīptāgni-vayaḥ-stha-bala-śālinām ।
virodhy api na pīḍāyai sātmyam alpaṃ ca bhojanam ।।

yāyāmi-snigdha-dīptāgni-
pādenā-pathyam abhyastaṃ pāda-pādena vā tyajet ।
niṣeveta hitaṃ tad-vad eka-dvi-try-antarī-kṛtam ।।

a-pathyam api hi tyaktaṃ śīlitaṃ pathyam eva vā ।
sātmyā-sātmya-vikārāya jāyate sahasānya-thā ।।

ātmyā-sātmyaṃ vikārāya
krameṇāpacitā doṣāḥ krameṇopacitā guṇāḥ ।
santo yānty a-punar-bhāvam a-prakampyā bhavanti ca ।।

āpnuvanti punar-bhāvam
aty-anta-saṃnidhānānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ dūṣaṇātmanām ।
a-hitair dūṣaṇaṃ bhūyo na vidvān kartum arhati ।।

āhāra-śayanā-brahma-caryair yuktyā prayojitaiḥ ।
śarīraṃ dhāryate nityam āgāram iva dhāraṇaiḥ ।।

-caryair yuktyā niṣevitaiḥ
āhāro varṇitas tatra tatra tatra ca vakṣyate ।
nidrāyattaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ puṣṭiḥ kārśyaṃ balā-balam ।।

atra tatra ca lakṣyate
vṛṣa-tā klība-tā jñānam a-jñānaṃ jīvitaṃ na ca ।
a-kāle ati-prasaṅgāc ca na ca nidrā niṣevitā ।।

sukhāyuṣī parākuryāt kāla-rātrir ivāparā ।
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ snigdhaṃ prasvapanaṃ divā ।।

a-rūkṣam an-abhiṣyandi tv āsīna-pracalāyitam ।
grīṣme vāyu-cayādāna-raukṣya-rātry-alpa-bhāvataḥ ।।

rīṣme vāta-cayādāna-
divā-svapno hito anyasmin kapha-pitta-karo hi saḥ ।
muktvā tu bhāṣya-yānādhva-madya-strī-bhāra-karmabhiḥ ।।

krodha-śoka-bhayaiḥ klāntān śvāsa-hidhmātisāriṇaḥ ।
vṛddha-bālā-bala-kṣīṇa-kṣata-tṛṭ-śūla-pīḍitān ।।

-kṣut-tṛṭ-śūla-nipīḍitān
a-jīrṇy-abhihatonmattān divā-svapnocitān api ।
dhātu-sāmyaṃ tathā hy eṣāṃ śleṣmā cāṅgāni puṣyati ।।

-jīrṇābhihatonmattān
bahu-medaḥ-kaphāḥ svapyuḥ sneha-nityāś ca nāhani ।
viṣārtaḥ kaṇṭha-rogī ca naiva jātu niśāsv api ।।

a-kāla-śayanān moha-jvara-staimitya-pīnasāḥ ।
śiro-ruk-śopha-hṛl-lāsa-sroto-rodhāgni-manda-tāḥ ।।

tatropavāsa-vamana-sveda-nāvanam auṣadham ।
yojayed ati-nidrāyāṃ tīkṣṇaṃ pracchardanāñjanam ।।

nāvanaṃ laṅghanaṃ cintāṃ vyavāyaṃ śoka-bhī-krudhaḥ ।
ebhir eva ca nidrāyā nāśaḥ śleṣmāti-saṃkṣayāt ।।

nidrā-nāśād aṅga-marda-śiro-gaurava-jṛmbhikāḥ ।
jāḍya-glāni-bhramā-pakti-tandrā rogāś ca vāta-jāḥ ।।

āḍyaṃ glāni-bhramā-pakti-
kapho alpo vāyunoddhūto dhamanīḥ saṃnirudhya tu ।
kuryāt saṃjñāpahāṃ tandrāṃ dāruṇāṃ moha-kāriṇīm ।।

unmīlita-vinirbhugne parivartita-tārake ।
bhavatas tatra nayane srute lulita-pakṣmaṇī ।।
ardha-tri-rātrāt sā sādhyā na sā sādhyā tataḥ param ।।
yathā-kālam ato nidrāṃ rātrau seveta sātmyataḥ ।
a-sātmyāj jāgarād ardhaṃ prātaḥ svapyād a-bhukta-vān ।।

-sātmya-jāgarād ardhaṃ
śīlayen manda-nidras tu kṣīra-madya-rasān dadhi ।
abhyaṅgodvartana-snāna-mūrdha-karṇākṣi-tarpaṇam ।।

kāntā-bāhu-latāśleṣo nirvṛtiḥ kṛta-kṛtya-tā ।
mano-'nukūlā viṣayāḥ kāmaṃ nidrā-sukha-pradāḥ ।।

brahma-carya-rater grāmya-sukha-niḥ-spṛha-cetasaḥ ।
nidrā saṃtoṣa-tṛptasya svaṃ kālaṃ nātivartate ।।

grāmya-dharme tyajen nārīm an-uttānāṃ rajasvalām ।
a-priyām a-priyācārāṃ duṣṭa-saṃkīrṇa-mehanām ।।

ati-sthūla-kṛśām sūtāṃ garbhiṇīm anya-yoṣitam ।
varṇinīm anya-yoniṃ ca guru-deva-nṛpālayam ।।

arbhiṇīm anya-yoṣitām
caitya-śmaśānāyatana-catvarāmbu-catuṣ-patham ।
parvāṇy an-aṅgaṃ divasaṃ śiro-hṛdaya-tāḍanam ।।

aty-āśito a-dhṛtiḥ kṣud-vān duḥ-sthitāṅgaḥ pipāsitaḥ ।
bālo vṛddho anya-vegārtas tyajed rogī ca maithunam ।।

seveta kāmataḥ kāmaṃ tṛpto vājī-kṛtām hime ।
try-ahād vasanta-śaradoḥ pakṣād varṣā-nidāghayoḥ ।।

ṛpto vājī-karair hime ṛpto vājī-kṛtair hime vy-ahād vasanta-śaradoḥ 
akṣād vṛṣṭi-nidāghayoḥ
bhrama-klamoru-daurbalya-bala-dhātv-indriya-kṣayāḥ ।
a-parva-maraṇaṃ ca syād anya-thā gacchataḥ striyam ।।

hrama-klamoru-daurbalyaṃ ala-dhātv-indriya-kṣayaḥ
smṛti-medhāyur-ārogya-puṣṭīndriya-yaśo-balaiḥ ।
adhikā manda-jaraso bhavanti strīṣu saṃyatāḥ ।।

havanti strīṣu saṃyutāḥ
snānānulepana-himānila-khaṇḍa-khādya-śītāmbu-dugdha-rasa-yūṣa-surā-prasannāḥ ।
seveta cānu śayanaṃ viratau ratasya tasyaivam āśu vapuṣaḥ punar eti dhāma ।।

śruta-carita-samṛddhe karma-dakṣe dayālau bhiṣaji nir-anubandhaṃ deha-rakṣāṃ niveśya । bhavati vipula-tejaḥ-svāsthya-kīrti-prabhāvaḥ sva-kuśala-phala-bhogī bhūmi-pālaś cirāyuḥ ।।

sūtrasthāna
mātrāśī sarva-kālaṃ syān mātrā hy agneḥ pravartikā ।
mātrāṃ dravyāṇy apekṣante gurūṇy api laghūny api ।।

gurūṇām ardha-sauhityaṃ laghūnāṃ nāti-tṛpta-tā ।
mātrā-pramāṇaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ sukhaṃ yāvad vijīryati ।।

ukhaṃ yāvad dhi jīryate
bhojanaṃ hīna-mātraṃ tu na balopacayaujase ।
sarveṣāṃ vāta-rogāṇāṃ hetu-tāṃ ca prapadyate ।।

ati-mātraṃ punaḥ sarvān āśu doṣān prakopayet ।
pīḍyamānā hi vātādyā yuga-pat tena kopitāḥ ।।

aṃpīḍyamānā vātādyā
āmenānnena duṣṭena tad evāviśya kurvate ।
viṣṭambhayanto alasakaṃ cyāvayanto viṣūcikām ।।

adharottara-mārgābhyāṃ sahasaivā-jitātmanaḥ ।
prayāti nordhvaṃ nādhas-tād āhāro na ca pacyate ।।

āmāśaye alasī-bhūtas tena so alasakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
vividhair vedanodbhedair vāyv-ādi-bhṛśa-kopataḥ ।।

sūcībhir iva gātrāṇi vidhyatīti viṣūcikā ।
tatra śūla-bhramānāha-kampa-stambhādayo anilāt ।।

pittāj jvarātisārāntar-dāha-tṛṭ-pralayādayaḥ ।
kaphāc chardy-aṅga-guru-tā-vāk-saṅga-ṣṭhīvanādayaḥ ।।

viśeṣād dur-balasyālpa-vahner vega-vidhāriṇaḥ ।
pīḍitaṃ mārutenānnaṃ śleṣmaṇā ruddham antarā ।।

alasaṃ kṣobhitaṃ doṣaiḥ śalya-tvenaiva saṃsthitam ।
śūlādīn kurute tīvrāṃś chardy-atīsāra-varjitān ।।

śalya-tveneva saṃsthitam
so alaso aty-artha-duṣṭās tu doṣā duṣṭāma-baddha-khāḥ ।
yāntas tiryak tanuṃ sarvāṃ daṇḍa-vat stambhayanti cet ।।

daṇḍakālasakaṃ nāma taṃ tyajed āśu-kāriṇam ।
viruddhādhyaśanā-jīrṇa-śīlino viṣa-lakṣaṇam ।।

āma-doṣaṃ mahā-ghoraṃ varjayed viṣa-saṃjñakam ।
viṣa-rūpāśu-kāri-tvād viruddhopakrama-tvataḥ ।।

athāmam alasī-bhūtaṃ sādhyaṃ tvaritam ullikhet ।
pītvā sogrā-paṭu-phalaṃ vāry uṣṇaṃ yojayet tataḥ ।।

svedanaṃ phala-vartiṃ ca mala-vātānulomanīm ।
nāmyamānāni cāṅgāni bhṛśaṃ svinnāni veṣṭayet ।।

ala-doṣānulomanīm
madanaṃ pippalī kuṣṭhaṃ vacā gaurāś ca sarṣapāḥ ।
guḍa-kṣāra-samāyuktā phala-vartiḥ praśasyate ।।

viṣūcyām ati-vṛddhāyāṃ pārṣṇyor dāhaḥ praśasyate ।
tad-ahaś copavāsyainaṃ virikta-vad upācaret ।।

tīvrārtir api nā-jīrṇī pibec chūla-ghnam auṣadham ।
āma-sanno analo nālaṃ paktuṃ doṣauṣadhāśanam ।।

nihanyād api caiteṣāṃ vibhramaḥ sahasāturam ।
jīrṇāśane tu bhaiṣajyaṃ yuñjyāt stabdha-gurūdare ।।

yāpattiḥ sahasāturam
doṣa-śeṣasya pākārtham agneḥ saṃdhukṣaṇāya ca ।
śāntir āma-vikārāṇāṃ bhavati tv apatarpaṇāt ।।

tri-vidhaṃ tri-vidhe doṣe tat samīkṣya prayojayet ।
tatrālpe laṅghanaṃ pathyaṃ madhye laṅghana-pācanam ।।

at samīkṣya prakalpayet
prabhūte śodhanaṃ tad dhi mūlād unmūlayen malān ।
evam anyān api vyādhīn sva-nidāna-viparyayāt ।।

cikitsed anubandhe tu sati hetu-viparyayam ।
tyaktvā yathā-yathaṃ vaidyo yuñjyād vyādhi-viparyayam ।।

tad-artha-kāri vā pakve doṣe tv iddhe ca pāvake ।
hitam abhyañjana-sneha-pāna-vasty-ādi yuktitaḥ ।।

oṣe vṛddhe ca pāvake oṣe tv ṛddhe tu pāvake
a-jīrṇaṃ ca kaphād āmaṃ tatra śopho akṣi-gaṇḍayoḥ ।
sadyo-bhukta ivodgāraḥ prasekotkleśa-gauravam ।।

viṣṭabdham anilāc chūla-vibandhādhmāna-sāda-kṛt ।
pittād vidagdhaṃ tṛṇ-moha-bhramāmlodgāra-dāha-vat ।।

-bhramāmlodgāra-dāha-kṛt
laṅghanaṃ kāryam āme tu viṣṭabdhe svedanaṃ bhṛśam ।
vidagdhe vamanaṃ yad vā yathāvasthaṃ hitaṃ bhavet ।।

athāvasthaṃ hitaṃ bhajet
garīyaso bhavel līnād āmād eva vilambikā ।
kapha-vātānubaddhāma-liṅgā tat-sama-sādhanā ।।

apha-vātānuviddhāma-
a-śraddhā hṛd-vyathā śuddhe apy udgāre rasa-śeṣataḥ ।
śayīta kiñ-cid evātra sarvaś cān-āśito divā ।।

arvaś cān-aśito divā
svapyād a-jīrṇī saṃjāta-bubhukṣo adyān mitaṃ laghu ।
vibandho ati-pravṛttir vā glānir māruta-mūḍha-tā ।।

lānir māruta-śūla-tā
a-jīrṇa-liṅgaṃ sāmānyaṃ viṣṭambho gauravaṃ bhramaḥ ।
na cāti-mātram evānnam āma-doṣāya kevalam ।।

dviṣṭa-viṣṭambhi-dagdhāma-guru-rūkṣa-himā-śuci ।
vidāhi śuṣkam aty-ambu-plutaṃ cānnaṃ na jīryati ।।

upataptena bhuktaṃ ca śoka-krodha-kṣud-ādibhiḥ ।
miśraṃ pathyam a-pathyaṃ ca bhuktaṃ samaśanaṃ matam ।।

śoka-krodha-kṣudhādibhiḥ rodha-śoka-bhayādibhiḥ
vidyād adhyaśanaṃ bhūyo bhuktasyopari bhojanam ।
a-kāle bahu cālpaṃ vā bhuktaṃ tu viṣamāśanam ।।

trīṇy apy etāni mṛtyuṃ vā ghorān vyādhīn sṛjanti vā ।
kāle sātmyaṃ śuci hitaṃ snigdhoṣṇaṃ laghu tan-manāḥ ।।

ṣaḍ-rasaṃ madhura-prāyaṃ nāti-druta-vilambitam ।
snātaḥ kṣud-vān vivikta-stho dhauta-pāda-karānanaḥ ।।

tarpayitvā pitṝn devān atithīn bālakān gurūn ।
pratyavekṣya tiraśco api pratipanna-parigrahān ।।

samīkṣya samyag ātmānam a-nindann a-bruvan dravam ।
iṣṭam iṣṭaiḥ sahāśnīyāc chuci-bhakta-janāhṛtam ।।

bhojanaṃ tṛṇa-keśādi-juṣṭam uṣṇī-kṛtaṃ punaḥ ।
śākāvarānna-bhūyiṣṭham aty-uṣṇa-lavaṇaṃ tyajet ।।

kilāṭa-dadhi-kūcīkā-kṣāra-śuktāma-mūlakam ।
kṛśa-śuṣka-varāhāvi-go-matsya-mahiṣāmiṣam ।।

-kṣāra-śuktāmla-mūlakam
māṣa-niṣpāva-śālūka-bisa-piṣṭa-virūḍhakam ।
śuṣka-śākāni yavakān phāṇitaṃ ca na śīlayet ।।

-tila-piṣṭa-virūḍhakam
śīlayec chāli-godhūma-yava-ṣaṣṭika-jāṅgalam ।
suniṣaṇṇaka-jīvantī-bāla-mūlaka-vāstukam ।।

pathyāmalaka-mṛdvīkā-paṭolī-mudga-śarkarāḥ ।
ghṛta-divyodaka-kṣīra-kṣaudra-dāḍima-saindhavam ।।

tri-phalāṃ madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ niśi netra-balāya ca ।
svāsthyānuvṛtti-kṛd yac ca rogoccheda-karaṃ ca yat ।।

bisekṣu-moca-cocāmra-modakotkārikādikam ।
adyād dravyaṃ guru snigdhaṃ svādu mandaṃ sthiraṃ puraḥ ।।

viparītam ataś cānte madhye amla-lavaṇotkaṭam ।
annena kukṣer dvāv aṃśau pānenaikaṃ prapūrayet ।।

āśrayaṃ pavanādīnāṃ caturtham avaśeṣayet ।
anu-pānaṃ himaṃ vāri yava-godhūmayor hitam ।।

dadhni madye viṣe kṣaudre koṣṇaṃ piṣṭa-mayeṣu tu ।
śāka-mudgādi-vikṛtau mastu-takrāmla-kāñjikam ।।

oṣṇaṃ piṣṭa-mayeṣu ca
surā kṛśānāṃ puṣṭy-arthaṃ sthūlānāṃ tu madhūdakam ।
śoṣe māṃsa-raso madyaṃ māṃse sv-alpe ca pāvake ।।

thūlānāṃ ca madhūdakam āṃseṣv alpe ca pāvake
vyādhy-auṣadhādhva-bhāṣya-strī-laṅghanātapa-karmabhiḥ ।
kṣīṇe vṛddhe ca bāle ca payaḥ pathyaṃ yathāmṛtam ।।

yādhy-auṣadhādhva-bhāra-strī-
viparītaṃ yad annasya guṇaiḥ syād a-virodhi ca ।
anu-pānaṃ samāsena sarva-dā tat praśasyate ।।

anu-pānaṃ karoty ūrjāṃ tṛptiṃ vyāptiṃ dṛḍhāṅga-tām ।
anna-saṃghāta-śaithilya-viklitti-jaraṇāni ca ।।

nordhva-jatru-gada-śvāsa-kāsoraḥ-kṣata-pīnase ।
gīta-bhāṣya-prasaṅge ca svara-bhede ca tad dhitam ।।

praklinna-deha-mehākṣi-gala-roga-vraṇāturāḥ ।
pānaṃ tyajeyuḥ sarvaś ca bhāṣyādhva-śayanaṃ tyajet ।।
pītvā bhuktvātapaṃ vahniṃ yānaṃ plavana-vāhanam ।।prasṛṣṭe viṇ-mūtre hṛdi su-vi-male doṣe sva-patha-ge ।।viśuddhe codgāre kṣud-upagamane vāte anusarati ।।tathāgnāv udrikte viśada-karaṇe dehe ca su-laghau ।।prayuñjītāhāraṃ vidhi-niyamitaṃ kālaḥ sa hi mataḥ ।।
rayuñjītāhāraṃ vidhi-niyamitaḥ kālaḥ sa hi mataḥ

sūtrasthāna
dravyam eva rasādīnāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ te hi tad-āśrayāḥ ।
pañca-bhūtātmakaṃ tat tu kṣmām adhiṣṭhāya jāyate ।।

ambu-yony-agni-pavana-nabhasām samavāyataḥ ।
tan-nirvṛttir viśeṣaś ca vyapadeśas tu bhūyasā ।।

yapadeśaś ca bhūyasā
tasmān naika-rasaṃ dravyaṃ bhūta-saṃghāta-saṃbhavāt ।
naika-doṣās tato rogās tatra vyakto rasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

an naika-bhūta-jaṃ dravyaṃ
a-vyakto anu-rasaḥ kiñ-cid ante vyakto api ceṣyate ।
gurv-ādayo guṇā dravye pṛthivy-ādau rasāśraye ।।

raseṣu vyapadiśyante sāhacaryopacārataḥ ।
tatra dravyaṃ guru-sthūla-sthira-gandha-guṇolbaṇam ।।

pārthivaṃ gaurava-sthairya-saṃghātopacayāvaham ।
drava-śīta-guru-snigdha-manda-sāndra-rasolbaṇam ।।

-manda-sāndra-guṇolbaṇam
āpyaṃ snehana-viṣyanda-kleda-prahlāda-bandha-kṛt ।
rūkṣa-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-viśada-sūkṣma-rūpa-guṇolbaṇam ।।

āgneyaṃ dāha-bhā-varṇa-prakāśa-pavanātmakam ।
vāyavyaṃ rūkṣa-viśada-laghu-sparśa-guṇolbaṇam ।।

raukṣya-lāghava-vaiśadya-vicāra-glāni-kārakam ।
nābhasaṃ sūkṣma-viśada-laghu-śabda-guṇolbaṇam ।।

-vicāra-glapanātmakam
sauṣirya-lāghava-karaṃ jagaty evam an-auṣadham ।
na kiñ-cid vidyate dravyaṃ vaśān nānārtha-yogayoḥ ।।

dravyam ūrdhva-gamaṃ tatra prāyo agni-pavanotkaṭam ।
adho-gāmi ca bhūyiṣṭhaṃ bhūmi-toya-guṇādhikam ।।

iti dravyaṃ rasān bhedair uttara-tropadekṣyate ।
vīryaṃ punar vadanty eke guru snigdhaṃ himaṃ mṛdu ।।

ti dravyaṃ raso bhedair
laghu rūkṣoṣṇa-tīkṣṇaṃ ca tad evaṃ matam aṣṭa-dhā ।
carakas tv āha vīryaṃ tat kriyate yena yā kriyā ।।

arakas tv āha vīryaṃ tu ena yā kriyate kriyā
nā-vīryaṃ kurute kiñ-cit sarvā vīrya-kṛtā hi sā ।
gurv-ādiṣv eva vīryākhyā tenānv-artheti varṇyate ।।

samagra-guṇa-sāreṣu śakty-utkarṣa-vivartiṣu ।
vyavahārāya mukhya-tvād bahv-agra-grahaṇād api ।।

amagra-guṇa-sāra-tvāc hakty-utkarṣa-vivartanāt
ataś ca viparīta-tvāt saṃbhavaty api naiva sā ।
vivakṣyate rasādyeṣu vīryaṃ gurv-ādayo hy ataḥ ।।

uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ dvi-dhaivānye vīryam ācakṣate api ca ।
nānātmakam api dravyam agnī-ṣomau mahā-balau ।।

vyaktā-vyaktaṃ jagad iva nātikrāmati jātu cit ।
tatroṣṇaṃ bhrama-tṛḍ-glāni-sveda-dāhāśu-pāki-tāḥ ।।

yaktā-vyaktaṃ jagad idaṃ yaktāvyaktaṃ yathā viśvaṃ
śamaṃ ca vāta-kaphayoḥ karoti śiśiraṃ punaḥ ।
hlādanaṃ jīvanaṃ stambhaṃ prasādaṃ rakta-pittayoḥ ।।

jāṭhareṇāgninā yogād yad udeti rasāntaram ।
rasānāṃ pariṇāmānte sa vipāka iti smṛtaḥ ।।

svāduḥ paṭuś ca madhuram amlo amlaṃ pacyate rasaḥ ।
tiktoṣaṇa-kaṣāyāṇāṃ vipākaḥ prāya-śaḥ kaṭuḥ ।।

rasair asau tulya-phalas tatra dravyaṃ śubhā-śubham ।
kiñ-cid rasena kurute karma pākena cāparam ।।

guṇāntareṇa vīryeṇa prabhāveṇaiva kiñ-ca-na ।
yad yad dravye rasādīnāṃ bala-vat-tvena vartate ।।

abhibhūyetarāṃs tat tat kāraṇa-tvaṃ prapadyate ।
viruddha-guṇa-saṃyoge bhūyasālpaṃ hi jīyate ।।

rasaṃ vipākas tau vīryaṃ prabhāvas tāny apohati ।
bala-sāmye rasādīnām iti naisargikaṃ balam ।।

rabhāvas tān vyapohati
rasādi-sāmye yat karma viśiṣṭaṃ tat prabhāva-jam ।
dantī rasādyais tulyāpi citrakasya virecanī ।।

madhukasya ca mṛdvīkā ghṛtaṃ kṣīrasya dīpanam ।
iti sāmānyataḥ karma dravyādīnāṃ punaś ca tat ।।

vicitra-pratyayārabdha-dravya-bhedena bhidyate ।
svādur guruś ca godhūmo vāta-jid vāta-kṛd yavaḥ ।।
uṣṇā matsyāḥ payaḥ śītaṃ kaṭuḥ siṃho na śūkaraḥ ।।
sūtrasthāna
kṣmāmbho-'gni-kṣmāmbu-tejaḥ-kha-vāyv-agny-anila-go-'nilaiḥ ।
dvayolbaṇaiḥ kramād bhūtair madhurādi-rasodbhavaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ vidyād rasaṃ svāduṃ yo vaktram anulimpati ।
āsvādyamāno dehasya hlādano akṣa-prasādanaḥ ।।

o vaktram upalimpati
priyaḥ pipīlikādīnām amlaḥ kṣālayate mukham ।
harṣaṇo roma-dantānām akṣi-bhruva-nikocanaḥ ।।

mlaḥ srāvayate mukham
lavaṇaḥ syandayaty āsyaṃ kapola-gala-dāha-kṛt ।
tikto viśadayaty āsyaṃ rasanaṃ pratihanti ca ।।

asanāṃ pratihanti ca
udvejayati jihvāgraṃ kurvaṃś cimicimāṃ kaṭuḥ ।
srāvayaty akṣi-nāsāsyaṃ kapolaṃ dahatīva ca ।।

kaṣāyo jaḍayej jihvāṃ kaṇṭha-sroto-vibandha-kṛt ।
rasānām iti rūpāṇi karmāṇi madhuro rasaḥ ।।

ā-janma-sātmyāt kurute dhātūnāṃ prabalaṃ balam ।
bāla-vṛddha-kṣata-kṣīṇa-varṇa-keśendriyaujasām ।।

praśasto bṛṃhaṇaḥ kaṇṭhyaḥ stanya-saṃdhāna-kṛd guruḥ ।
āyuṣyo jīvanaḥ snigdhaḥ pittānila-viṣāpahaḥ ।।

kurute aty-upayogena sa medaḥ-śleṣma-jān gadān ।
sthaulyāgni-sāda-saṃnyāsa-meha-gaṇḍārbudādikān ।।

a medaḥ-kapha-jān gadān
amlo agni-dīpti-kṛt snigdho hṛdyaḥ pācana-rocanaḥ ।
uṣṇa-vīryo hima-sparśaḥ prīṇanaḥ kledano laghuḥ ।।

ṣṇa-vīryo himaḥ sparśe rīṇano bhedano laghuḥ
karoti kapha-pittāsraṃ mūḍha-vātānulomanaḥ ।
so aty-abhyastas tanoḥ kuryāc chaithilyaṃ timiraṃ bhramam ।।

ūḍha-vātānulomanam
kaṇḍū-pāṇḍu-tva-vīsarpa-śopha-visphoṭa-tṛḍ-jvarān ।
lavaṇaḥ stambha-saṃghāta-bandha-vidhmāpano agni-kṛt ।।

snehanaḥ svedanas tīkṣṇo rocanaś cheda-bheda-kṛt ।
so ati-yukto asra-pavanaṃ khalatiṃ palitaṃ valīm ।।

tṛṭ-kuṣṭha-viṣa-vīsarpān janayet kṣapayed balam ।
tiktaḥ svayam a-rociṣṇur a-ruciṃ kṛmi-tṛḍ-viṣam ।।

kuṣṭha-mūrchā-jvarotkleśa-dāha-pitta-kaphāñ jayet ।
kleda-medo-vasā-majja-śakṛn-mūtropaśoṣaṇaḥ ।।

laghur medhyo himo rūkṣaḥ stanya-kaṇṭha-viśodhanaḥ ।
dhātu-kṣayānila-vyādhīn ati-yogāt karoti saḥ ।।

hātu-kṣayaṃ cala-vyādhīn
kaṭur galāmayodarda-kuṣṭhālasaka-śopha-jit ।
vraṇāvasādanaḥ sneha-medaḥ-kledopaśoṣaṇaḥ ।।

dīpanaḥ pācano rucyaḥ śodhano annasya śoṣaṇaḥ ।
chinatti bandhān srotāṃsi vivṛṇoti kaphāpahaḥ ।।

śodhano annasya hāṣaṇaḥ
kurute so ati-yogena tṛṣṇāṃ śukra-bala-kṣayam ।
mūrchām ākuñcanaṃ kampaṃ kaṭī-pṛṣṭhādiṣu vyathām ।।

urute so ati-vegena
kaṣāyaḥ pitta-kapha-hā gurur asra-viśodhanaḥ ।
pīḍano ropaṇaḥ śītaḥ kleda-medo-viśoṣaṇaḥ ।।

āma-saṃstambhano grāhī rūkṣo ati tvak-prasādanaḥ ।
karoti śīlitaḥ so ati viṣṭambhādhmāna-hṛd-rujaḥ ।।

tṛṭ-kārśya-pauruṣa-bhraṃśa-sroto-rodha-mala-grahān ।
ghṛta-hema-guḍākṣoṭa-moca-coca-parūṣakam ।।

-sroto-rodha-gala-grahān -sroto-bandha-mala-grahān
abhīru-vīrā-panasa-rājādana-balā-trayam ।
mede catasraḥ parṇinyo jīvantī jīvakarṣabhau ।।

madhūkaṃ madhukaṃ bimbī vidārī śrāvaṇī-yugam ।
kṣīraśuklā tukākṣīrī kṣīriṇyau kāśmarī sahe ।।

ṣīraśuklā tavakṣīrī
kṣīrekṣu-gokṣura-kṣaudra-drākṣādir madhuro gaṇaḥ ।
amlo dhātrī-phalāmlīkā-mātuluṅgāmla-vetasam ।।

dāḍimaṃ rajataṃ takraṃ cukraṃ pālevataṃ dadhi ।
āmram āmrātakaṃ bhavyaṃ kapitthaṃ karamardakam ।।

vṛkṣāmla-kola-likuca-kośāmlātaka-dhanvanam ।
mastu-dhānyāmla-madyāni jambīraṃ tila-kaṇṭakam ।।

varaṃ sauvarcalaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ viḍaṃ sāmudram audbhidam ।
romakaṃ pāṃsu-jaṃ sīsaṃ kṣāraś ca lavaṇo gaṇaḥ ।।

ṣārāś ca lavaṇo gaṇaḥ
tiktaḥ paṭolī trāyantī vālakośīra-candanam ।
bhūnimba-nimba-kaṭukā-tagarāguru-vatsakam ।।

naktamāla-dvi-rajanī-musta-mūrvāṭarūṣakam ।
pāṭhāpāmārga-kāṃsyāyo-guḍūcī-dhanvayāsakam ।।

pañca-mūlaṃ mahad vyāghryau viśālātiviṣā vacā ।
kaṭuko hiṅgu-marica-kṛmijit-pañca-kolakam ।।

aṭuko hiṅgu-maricaṃ ṛmijit-pañca-kolakam
kuṭherādyā haritakāḥ pittaṃ mūtram aruṣkaram ।
vargaḥ kaṣāyaḥ pathyākṣaṃ śirīṣaḥ khadiro madhu ।।

ittaṃ mūtram aruṣkaraḥ argaḥ kaṣāyaḥ pathyākṣaḥ
kadambodumbaraṃ muktā-pravālāñjana-gairikam ।
bālaṃ kapitthaṃ kharjūraṃ bisa-padmotpalādi ca ।।

isa-padmotpalāni ca
madhuraṃ śleṣmalaṃ prāyo jīrṇāc chāli-yavād ṛte ।
mudgād godhūmataḥ kṣaudrāt sitāyā jāṅgalāmiṣāt ।।

prāyo amlaṃ pitta-jananaṃ dāḍimāmalakād ṛte ।
a-pathyaṃ lavaṇaṃ prāyaś cakṣuṣo anya-tra saindhavāt ।।

tiktaṃ kaṭu ca bhūyiṣṭham a-vṛṣyaṃ vāta-kopanam ।
ṛte amṛtā-paṭolībhyāṃ śuṇṭhī-kṛṣṇā-rasonataḥ ।।

kaṣāyaṃ prāya-śaḥ śītaṃ stambhanaṃ cābhayāṃ vinā ।
rasāḥ kaṭv-amla-lavaṇā vīryeṇoṣṇā yathottaram ।।

tambhanaṃ cābhayāmṛte
tiktaḥ kaṣāyo madhuras tad-vad eva ca śītalāḥ ।
tiktaḥ kaṭuḥ kaṣāyaś ca rūkṣā baddha-malās tathā ।।

paṭv-amla-madhurāḥ snigdhāḥ sṛṣṭa-viṇ-mūtra-mārutāḥ ।
paṭoḥ kaṣāyas tasmāc ca madhuraḥ paramaṃ guruḥ ।।

laghur amlaḥ kaṭus tasmāt tasmād api ca tiktakaḥ ।
saṃyogāḥ sapta-pañcāśat kalpanā tu tri-ṣaṣṭi-dhā ।।

lavaṇād amla-madhurau kāryau syātāṃ yathā-kramam ।
vāyor nir-anubandhasya pāka-śānti-pravṛttaye ।।

āka-śānti-prasaktaye
prāk tikto madhuraḥ paścāt kaṣāyo ante vidhīyate ।
taiḥ pittaṃ śamam abhyeti pakvācchī-kṛta-piṇḍitam ।।

kaṭuḥ prāk tiktakaḥ paścāt kaṣāyo ante vidhīyate ।
taiḥ śleṣmā śamam abhyeti pakvācchī-kṛta-piṇḍitaḥ ।।

aṭukaḥ prāk tatas tiktaḥ akvo acchī-kṛta-piṇḍitaḥ
rasānāṃ yaugika-tvena yathā-sthūlaṃ vibhajyate ।
ekaika-hīnās tān pañca-daśa yānti rasā dvike ।।

kaika-hīnās te pañca- -pañca yānti rasā dvike
svādur dvikeṣu pañcāmlaś caturo lavaṇas trayam ।
dvau tiktaḥ kaṭukaś caikaṃ yāti pañca-daśeti tu ।।

trike svādur daśāmlaḥ ṣaṭ trīn paṭus tikta ekakam ।
catuṣkeṣu daśa svāduś caturo amlaḥ paṭuḥ sakṛt ।।

atuṣke tu daśa svāduś
pañcakeṣv ekam evāmlo madhuraḥ pañca sevate ।
dravyam ekaṃ ṣaḍ-āsvādam a-saṃyuktāś ca ṣaḍ rasāḥ ।।

ṣaṭ pañcakā ṣaṭ ca pṛthag rasāḥ syuś catur-dvikau pañca-daśa-prakārau ।
bhedās trikā viṃśatir ekam eva dravyaṃ ṣaḍ-āsvādam iti tri-ṣaṣṭiḥ ।।

te rasānu-rasato rasa-bhedās tāratamya-parikalpanayā ca ।
saṃbhavanti gaṇanāṃ samatītā doṣa-bheṣaja-vaśād upayojyāḥ ।।

sūtrasthāna
doṣa-dhātu-malā mūlaṃ sadā dehasya taṃ calaḥ ।
utsāhocchvāsa-niśvāsa-ceṣṭā-vega-pravartanaiḥ ।।

samyag-gatyā ca dhātūnām akṣāṇāṃ pāṭavena ca ।
anugṛhṇāty a-vikṛtaḥ pittaṃ pakty-ūṣma-darśanaiḥ ।।

kṣut-tṛḍ-ruci-prabhā-medhā-dhī-śaurya-tanu-mārdavaiḥ ।
śleṣmā sthira-tva-snigdha-tva-saṃdhi-bandha-kṣamādibhiḥ ।।

prīṇanaṃ jīvanaṃ lepaḥ sneho dhāraṇa-pūraṇe ।
garbhotpādaś ca dhātūnāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ karma kramāt smṛtam ।।

avaṣṭambhaḥ purīṣasya mūtrasya kleda-vāhanam ।
svedasya kleda-vidhṛtir vṛddhas tu kurute anilaḥ ।।

vedasya keśa-vidhṛtir ṛddhaś ca kurute anilaḥ
kārśya-kārṣṇyoṣṇa-kāma-tva-kampānāha-śakṛd-grahān ।
bala-nidrendriya-bhraṃśa-pralāpa-bhrama-dīna-tāḥ ।।

ārśya-kārṣṇyoṣṇa-kāmi-tva-
pīta-viṇ-mūtra-netra-tvak-kṣut-tṛḍ-dāhālpa-nidra-tāḥ ।
pittaṃ śleṣmāgni-sadana-prasekālasya-gauravam ।।

śvaitya-śaitya-ślathāṅga-tvaṃ śvāsa-kāsāti-nidra-tāḥ ।
raso api śleṣma-vad raktaṃ visarpa-plīha-vidradhīn ।।

kuṣṭha-vātāsra-pittāsra-gulmopa-kuśa-kāmalāḥ ।
vyaṅgāgni-nāśa-saṃmoha-rakta-tvaṅ-netra-mūtra-tāḥ ।।

yaṅgāgni-sāda-saṃmoha
māṃsaṃ gaṇḍārbuda-granthi-gaṇḍorūdara-vṛddhi-tāḥ ।
kaṇṭhādiṣv adhi-māṃsaṃ ca tad-van medas tathā śramam ।।

-gaṇḍorūdara-vṛddha-tāḥ
alpe api ceṣṭite śvāsaṃ sphik-stanodara-lambanam ।
asthy adhy-asthy adhi-dantāṃś ca majjā netrāṅga-gauravam ।।

ūtraṃ tu vaster nistodaṃ
parvasu sthūla-mūlāni kuryāt kṛcchrāṇy arūṃṣi ca ।
ati-strī-kāma-tāṃ vṛddhaṃ śuktaṃ śukrāśmarīm api ।।

kukṣāv ādhmānam āṭopaṃ gauravaṃ vedanāṃ śakṛt ।
mūtraṃ tu vasti-nistodaṃ kṛte apy a-kṛta-saṃjña-tām ।।

svedo ati-sveda-daurgandhya-kaṇḍūr evaṃ ca lakṣayet ।
dūṣikādīn api malān bāhulya-guru-tādibhiḥ ।।

liṅgaṃ kṣīṇe anile aṅgasya sādo alpaṃ bhāṣitehitam ।
saṃjñā-mohas tathā śleṣma-vṛddhy-uktāmaya-saṃbhavaḥ ।।

pitte mando analaḥ śītaṃ prabhā-hāniḥ kaphe bhramaḥ ।
śleṣmāśayānāṃ śūnya-tvaṃ hṛd-dravaḥ ślatha-saṃdhi-tā ।।

ṛd-gadaḥ ślatha-saṃdhi-tā
rase raukṣyaṃ śramaḥ śoṣo glāniḥ śabdā-sahiṣṇu-tā ।
rakte amla-śiśira-prīti-sirā-śaithilya-rūkṣa-tāḥ ।।

māṃse akṣa-glāni-gaṇḍa-sphik-śuṣka-tā-saṃdhi-vedanāḥ ।
medasi svapanaṃ kaṭyāḥ plīhno vṛddhiḥ kṛśāṅga-tā ।।

asthny asthi-todaḥ śadanaṃ danta-keśa-nakhādiṣu ।
asthnāṃ majjani sauṣiryaṃ bhramas timira-darśanam ।।

sthny asthi-todaḥ sadanaṃ
śukre cirāt prasicyeta śukraṃ śoṇitam eva vā ।
todo aty-arthaṃ vṛṣaṇayor meḍhraṃ dhūmāyatīva ca ।।

purīṣe vāyur antrāṇi sa-śabdo veṣṭayann iva ।
kukṣau bhramati yāty ūrdhvaṃ hṛt-pārśve pīḍayan bhṛśam ।।

ukṣiṃ bhramati yāty ūrdhvaṃ
mūtre alpaṃ mūtrayet kṛcchrād vi-varṇaṃ sāsram eva vā ।
svede roma-cyutiḥ stabdha-roma-tā sphuṭanaṃ tvacaḥ ।।

malānām ati-sūkṣmāṇāṃ dur-lakṣyaṃ lakṣayet kṣayam ।
sva-malāyana-saṃśoṣa-toda-śūnya-tva-lāghavaiḥ ।।

doṣādīnāṃ yathā-svaṃ ca vidyād vṛddhi-kṣayau bhiṣak ।
kṣayeṇa viparītānāṃ guṇānāṃ vardhanena ca ।।

vṛddhiṃ malānāṃ saṅgāc ca kṣayaṃ cāti-visargataḥ ।
malocita-tvād dehasya kṣayo vṛddhes tu pīḍanaḥ ।।

tatrāsthani sthito vāyuḥ pittaṃ tu sveda-raktayoḥ ।
śleṣmā śeṣeṣu tenaiṣām āśrayāśrayiṇāṃ mithaḥ ।।

yad ekasya tad anyasya vardhana-kṣapaṇauṣadham ।
asthi-mārutayor naivaṃ prāyo vṛddhir hi tarpaṇāt ।।

śleṣmaṇānugatā tasmāt saṃkṣayas tad-viparyayāt ।
vāyunānugato asmāc ca vṛddhi-kṣaya-samudbhavān ।।

vikārān sādhayec chīghraṃ kramāl laṅghana-bṛṃhaṇaiḥ ।
vāyor anya-tra taj-jāṃs tu tair evotkrama-yojitaiḥ ।।

viśeṣād rakta-vṛddhy-utthān rakta-sruti-virecanaiḥ ।
māṃsa-vṛddhi-bhavān rogān śastra-kṣārāgni-karmabhiḥ ।।

sthaulya-kārśyopacāreṇa medo-jān asthi-saṃkṣayāt ।
jātān kṣīra-ghṛtais tikta-saṃyutair vastibhis tathā ।।

-saṃyuktair vastibhis tathā
majja-śukrodbhavān rogān bhojanaiḥ svādu-tiktakaiḥ ।
vṛddhaṃ śukraṃ vyavāyādyair yac cānyac chukra-śoṣikam ।।

raty-anīkauṣadhaṃ majja- -śukra-vṛddhi-kṣaye hitam
viḍ-vṛddhi-jān atīsāra-kriyayā viṭ-kṣayodbhavān ।
meṣāja-madhya-kulmāṣa-yava-māṣa-dvayādibhiḥ ।।

mūtra-vṛddhi-kṣayotthāṃś ca meha-kṛcchra-cikitsayā ।
vyāyāmābhyañjana-sveda-madyaiḥ sveda-kṣayodbhavān ।।

ūtra-vṛddhi-kṣayotthāṃs tu
sva-sthāna-sthasya kāyāgner aṃśā dhātuṣu saṃśritāḥ ।
teṣāṃ sādāti-dīptibhyāṃ dhātu-vṛddhi-kṣayodbhavaḥ ।।

pūrvo dhātuḥ paraṃ kuryād vṛddhaḥ kṣīṇaś ca tad-vidham ।
doṣā duṣṭā rasair dhātūn dūṣayanty ubhaye malān ।।
