adho dve sapta śirasi khāni sveda-vahāni ca ।
malā malāyanāni syur yathā-svaṃ teṣv ato gadāḥ ।।

ojas tu tejo dhātūnāṃ śukrāntānāṃ paraṃ smṛtam ।
hṛdaya-stham api vyāpi deha-sthiti-nibandhanam ।।

snigdhaṃ somātmakaṃ śuddham īṣal-lohita-pītakam ।
yan-nāśe niyataṃ nāśo yasmiṃs tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhati ।।

niṣpadyante yato bhāvā vividhā deha-saṃśrayāḥ ।
ojaḥ kṣīyeta kopa-kṣud-dhyāna-śoka-śramādibhiḥ ।।

bibheti dur-balo abhīkṣṇaṃ dhyāyati vyathitendriyaḥ ।
duś-chāyo dur-manā rūkṣo bhavet kṣāmaś ca tat-kṣaye ।।

i-cchāyo dur-manā rūkṣo havet kṣāmaś ca tat-kṣayāt
jīvanīyauṣadha-kṣīra-rasādyās tatra bheṣajam ।
ojo-vṛddhau hi dehasya tuṣṭi-puṣṭi-balodayaḥ ।।

jo-vṛddhau ca dehasya jo-vṛddhau tu dehasya 
tuṣṭi-puṣṭi-balodayāḥ
yad annaṃ dveṣṭi yad api prārthayetā-virodhi tu ।
tat tat tyajan samaśnaṃś ca tau tau vṛddhi-kṣayau jayet ।।

at tat tyajan samaśnan vā
kurvate hi ruciṃ doṣā viparīta-samānayoḥ ।
vṛddhāḥ kṣīṇāś ca bhūyiṣṭhaṃ lakṣayanty a-budhās tu na ।।

urvanti hi ruciṃ doṣā
yathā-balaṃ yathā-svaṃ ca doṣā vṛddhā vitanvate ।
rūpāṇi jahati kṣīṇāḥ samāḥ svaṃ karma kurvate ।।

ya eva dehasya samā vivṛddhyai ta eva doṣā viṣamā vadhāya ।
yasmād atas te hita-caryayaiva kṣayād vivṛddher iva rakṣaṇīyāḥ ।।

ṣayād vivṛddher api rakṣaṇīyāḥ

sūtrasthāna
pakvāśaya-kaṭī-sakthi-śrotrāsthi-sparśanendriyam ।
sthānaṃ vātasya tatrāpi pakvādhānaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

nābhir āmāśayaḥ svedo lasīkā rudhiraṃ rasaḥ ।
dṛk sparśanaṃ ca pittasya nābhir atra viśeṣataḥ ।।

uraḥ-kaṇṭha-śiraḥ-kloma-parvāṇy āmāśayo rasaḥ ।
medo ghrāṇaṃ ca jihvā ca kaphasya su-tarām uraḥ ।।

prāṇādi-bhedāt pañcātmā vāyuḥ prāṇo atra mūrdha-gaḥ ।
uraḥ-kaṇṭha-caro buddhi-hṛdayendriya-citta-dhṛk ।।

ṣṭhīvana-kṣavathūdgāra-niḥśvāsānna-praveśa-kṛt ।
uraḥ sthānam udānasya nāsā-nābhi-galāṃś caret ।।

āsā-nābhi-galāṃś caran
vāk-pravṛtti-prayatnorjā-bala-varṇa-smṛti-kriyaḥ ।
vyāno hṛdi sthitaḥ kṛtsna-deha-cārī mahā-javaḥ ।।

gaty-apakṣepaṇotkṣepa-nimeṣonmeṣaṇādikāḥ ।
prāyaḥ sarvāḥ kriyās tasmin pratibaddhāḥ śarīriṇām ।।

samāno agni-samīpa-sthaḥ koṣṭhe carati sarvataḥ ।
annaṃ gṛhṇāti pacati vivecayati muñcati ।।

apāno apāna-gaḥ śroṇi-vasti-meḍhroru-go-caraḥ ।
śukrārtava-śakṛn-mūtra-garbha-niṣkramaṇa-kriyaḥ ।।

pittaṃ pañcātmakaṃ tatra pakvāmāśaya-madhya-gam ।
pañca-bhūtātmaka-tve api yat taijasa-guṇodayāt ।।

tyakta-dravya-tvaṃ pākādi-karmaṇānala-śabditam ।
pacaty annaṃ vibhajate sāra-kiṭṭau pṛthak tathā ।।

āra-kiṭṭe pṛthak tathā
tatra-stham eva pittānāṃ śeṣāṇām apy anugraham ।
karoti bala-dānena pācakaṃ nāma tat smṛtam ।।

āmāśayāśrayaṃ pittaṃ rañjakaṃ rasa-rañjanāt ।
buddhi-medhābhimānādyair abhipretārtha-sādhanāt ।।

sādhakaṃ hṛd-gataṃ pittaṃ rūpālocanataḥ smṛtam ।
dṛk-stham ālocakaṃ tvak-sthaṃ bhrājakaṃ bhrājanāt tvacaḥ ।।

śleṣmā tu pañca-dhoraḥ-sthaḥ sa trikasya sva-vīryataḥ ।
hṛdayasyānna-vīryāc ca tat-stha evāmbu-karmaṇā ।।

śleṣmāpi pañca-dhoraḥ-sthaḥ
kapha-dhāmnāṃ ca śeṣāṇāṃ yat karoty avalambanam ।
ato avalambakaḥ śleṣmā yas tv āmāśaya-saṃsthitaḥ ।।

as tv āmāśaya-saṃśritaḥ
kledakaḥ so anna-saṃghāta-kledanād rasa-bodhanāt ।
bodhako rasanā-sthāyī śiraḥ-saṃstho akṣa-tarpaṇāt ।।

tarpakaḥ saṃdhi-saṃśleṣāc chleṣakaḥ saṃdhiṣu sthitaḥ ।
iti prāyeṇa doṣāṇāṃ sthānāny a-vikṛtātmanām ।।

hleṣakaḥ saṃdhi-saṃsthitaḥ
vyāpinām api jānīyāt karmāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak ।
uṣṇena yuktā rūkṣādyā vāyoḥ kurvanti saṃcayam ।।

śītena kopam uṣṇena śamaṃ snigdhādayo guṇāḥ ।
śītena yuktās tīkṣṇādyāś cayaṃ pittasya kurvate ।।

uṣṇena kopaṃ mandādyāḥ śamaṃ śītopasaṃhitāḥ ।
śītena yuktāḥ snigdhādyāḥ kurvate śleṣmaṇaś cayam ।।

uṣṇena kopaṃ tenaiva guṇā rūkṣādayaḥ śamam ।
cayo vṛddhiḥ sva-dhāmny eva pradveṣo vṛddhi-hetuṣu ।।

viparīta-guṇecchā ca kopas tūn-mārga-gami-tā ।
liṅgānāṃ darśanaṃ sveṣām a-svāsthyaṃ roga-saṃbhavaḥ ।।

sva-sthāna-sthasya sama-tā vikārā-saṃbhavaḥ śamaḥ ।
caya-prakopa-praśamā vāyor grīṣmādiṣu triṣu ।।

varṣādiṣu tu pittasya śleṣmaṇaḥ śiśirādiṣu ।
cīyate laghu-rūkṣābhir oṣadhibhiḥ samīraṇaḥ ।।

arṣādiṣu ca pittasya
tad-vidhas tad-vidhe dehe kālasyauṣṇyān na kupyati ।
adbhir amla-vipākābhir oṣadhibhiś ca tādṛśam ।।

pittaṃ yāti cayaṃ kopaṃ na tu kālasya śaityataḥ ।
cīyate snigdha-śītābhir udakauṣadhibhiḥ kaphaḥ ।।

tulye api kāle dehe ca skanna-tvān na prakupyati ।
iti kāla-sva-bhāvo ayam āhārādi-vaśāt punaḥ ।।

kanna-tvān na vikupyati
cayādīn yānti sadyo api doṣāḥ kāle api vā na tu ।
vyāpnoti sahasā deham ā-pāda-tala-mastakam ।।

nivartate tu kupito malo alpālpaṃ jalaugha-vat ।
nānā-rūpair a-saṃkhyeyair vikāraiḥ kupitā malāḥ ।।

tāpayanti tanuṃ tasmāt tad-dhetv-ākṛti-sādhanam ।
śakyaṃ naikaika-śo vaktum ataḥ sāmānyam ucyate ।।

doṣā eva hi sarveṣāṃ rogāṇām eka-kāraṇam ।
yathā pakṣī paripatan sarvataḥ sarvam apy ahaḥ ।।

chāyām atyeti nātmīyāṃ yathā vā kṛtsnam apy adaḥ ।
vikāra-jātaṃ vividhaṃ trīn guṇān nātivartate ।।

tathā sva-dhātu-vaiṣamya-nimittam api sarva-dā ।
vikāra-jātaṃ trīn doṣān teṣāṃ kope tu kāraṇam ।।

arthair a-sātmyaiḥ saṃyogaḥ kālaḥ karma ca duṣ-kṛtam ।
hīnāti-mithyā-yogena bhidyate tat punas tri-dhā ।।

hīno arthenendriyasyālpaḥ saṃyogaḥ svena naiva vā ।
ati-yogo ati-saṃsargaḥ sūkṣma-bhāsura-bhairavam ।।

aty-āsannāti-dūra-sthaṃ vi-priyaṃ vikṛtādi ca ।
yad akṣṇā vīkṣyate rūpaṃ mithyā-yogaḥ sa dāruṇaḥ ।।

ithyā-yogaḥ su-dāruṇaḥ
evam aty-ucca-pūty-ādīn indriyārthān yathā-yatham ।
vidyāt kālas tu śītoṣṇa-varṣā-bhedāt tri-dhā mataḥ ।।

-varṣa-bhedāt tri-dhā mataḥ
sa hīno hīna-śītādir ati-yogo ati-lakṣaṇaḥ ।
mithyā-yogas tu nirdiṣṭo viparīta-sva-lakṣaṇaḥ ।।

kāya-vāk-citta-bhedena karmāpi vibhajet tri-dhā ।
kāyādi-karmaṇo hīnā pravṛttir hīna-saṃjñakaḥ ।।

āyādi-karmaṇāṃ hīnā ravṛttir hīna-saṃjñikā
ati-yogo ati-vṛttis tu vegodīraṇa-dhāraṇam ।
viṣamāṅga-kriyārambha-patana-skhalanādikam ।।

ti-yogo ati-vṛttiś ca
bhāṣaṇaṃ sāmi-bhuktasya rāga-dveṣa-bhayādi ca ।
karma prāṇātipātādi daśa-dhā yac ca ninditam ।।

mithyā-yogaḥ samasto asāv iha vāmu-tra vā kṛtam ।
nidānam etad doṣāṇāṃ kupitās tena naika-dhā ।।

ha cāmu-tra vā kṛtam
kurvanti vividhān vyādhīn śākhā-koṣṭhāsthi-saṃdhiṣu ।
śākhā raktādayas tvak ca bāhya-rogāyanaṃ hi tat ।।

āhya-rogāyanaṃ hi sā
tad-āśrayā maṣa-vyaṅga-gaṇḍālajy-arbudādayaḥ ।
bahir-bhāgāś ca dur-nāma-gulma-śophādayo gadāḥ ।।

antaḥ koṣṭho mahā-srota āma-pakvāśayāśrayaḥ ।
tat-sthānāḥ chardy-atīsāra-kāsa-śvāsodara-jvarāḥ ।।

antar-bhāgaṃ ca śophārśo-gulma-visarpa-vidradhi ।
śiro-hṛdaya-vasty-ādi-marmāṇy asthnāṃ ca saṃdhayaḥ ।।

-marmāṇy asthnāṃ tu saṃdhayaḥ
tan-nibaddhāḥ sirā-snāyu-kaṇḍarādyāś ca madhyamaḥ ।
roga-mārgaḥ sthitās tatra yakṣma-pakṣa-vadhārditāḥ ।।

mūrdhādi-rogāḥ saṃdhy-asthi-trika-śūla-grahādayaḥ ।
sraṃsa-vyāsa-vyadha-svāp a-sāda-ruk-toda-bhedanam ।।

saṅgāṅga-bhaṅga-saṃkoca-varta-harṣaṇa-tarpaṇam ।
kampa-pāruṣya-sauṣirya-śoṣa-spandana-veṣṭanam ।।

stambhaḥ kaṣāya-rasa-tā varṇaḥ śyāvo aruṇo api vā ।
karmāṇi vāyoḥ pittasya dāha-rāgoṣma-pāki-tāḥ ।।

svedaḥ kledaḥ srutiḥ kothaḥ sadanaṃ mūrchanaṃ madaḥ ।
kaṭukāmlau rasau varṇaḥ pāṇḍurāruṇa-varjitaḥ ।।

śleṣmaṇaḥ sneha-kāṭhinya-kaṇḍū-śīta-tva-gauravam ।
bandhopalepa-staimitya-śophā-pakty-ati-nidra-tāḥ ।।

varṇaḥ śveto rasau svādu-lavaṇau cira-kāri-tā ।
ity a-śeṣāmaya-vyāpi yad uktaṃ doṣa-lakṣaṇam ।।

darśanādyair avahitas tat samyag upalakṣayet ।
vyādhy-avasthā-vibhāga-jñaḥ paśyann ārtān prati-kṣaṇam ।।

abhyāsāt prāpyate dṛṣṭiḥ karma-siddhi-prakāśinī ।
ratnādi-sad-a-saj-jñānaṃ na śāstrād eva jāyate ।।

bhyāsāj jāyate dṛṣṭiḥ bhyāsāt kevalaṃ dṛṣṭiḥ
dṛṣṭāpacāra-jaḥ kaś-cit kaś-cit pūrvāparādha-jaḥ ।
tat-saṃkarād bhavaty anyo vyādhir evaṃ tri-dhā smṛtaḥ ।।

aś-cit pūrvāpacāra-jaḥ yādhir evaṃ tri-dhā mataḥ
yathā-nidānaṃ doṣotthaḥ karma-jo hetubhir vinā ।
mahārambho alpake hetāv ātaṅko doṣa-karma-jaḥ ।।

vipakṣa-śīlanāt pūrvaḥ karma-jaḥ karma-saṃkṣayāt ।
gacchaty ubhaya-janmā tu doṣa-karma-kṣayāt kṣayam ।।

dvi-dhā sva-para-tantra-tvād vyādhayo antyāḥ punar dvi-dhā ।
pūrva-jāḥ pūrva-rūpākhyā jātāḥ paścād upadravāḥ ।।

yathā-sva-janmopaśayāḥ sva-tantrāḥ spaṣṭa-lakṣaṇāḥ ।
viparītās tato anye tu vidyād evaṃ malān api ।।

tāō̃ lakṣayed avahito vikurvāṇān prati-jvaram ।
teṣāṃ pradhāna-praśame praśamo a-śāmyatas tathā ।।

paścāc cikitset tūrṇaṃ vā bala-vantam upadravam ।
vyādhi-kliṣṭa-śarīrasya pīḍā-kara-taro hi saḥ ।।

aścāc cikitset pūrvaṃ vā
vikāra-nāmā-kuśalo na jihrīyāt kadā-ca-na ।
na hi sarva-vikārāṇāṃ nāmato asti dhruvā sthitiḥ ।।

sa eva kupito doṣaḥ samutthāna-viśeṣataḥ ।
sthānāntarāṇi ca prāpya vikārān kurute bahūn ।।

tasmād vikāra-prakṛtīr adhiṣṭhānāntarāṇi ca ।
buddhvā hetu-viśeṣāṃś ca śīghraṃ kuryād upakramam ।।

dūṣyaṃ deśaṃ balaṃ kālam analaṃ prakṛtiṃ vayaḥ ।
sat-tvaṃ sātmyaṃ tathāhāram avasthāś ca pṛthag-vidhāḥ ।।

sūkṣma-sūkṣmāḥ samīkṣyaiṣāṃ doṣauṣadha-nirūpaṇe ।
yo vartate cikitsāyāṃ na sa skhalati jātu cit ।।

gurv-alpa-vyādhi-saṃsthānaṃ sat-tva-deha-balā-balāt ।
dṛśyate apy anya-thā-kāraṃ tasminn avahito bhavet ।।

guruṃ laghum iti vyādhiṃ kalpayaṃs tu bhiṣag-bruvaḥ ।
alpa-doṣākalanayā pathye vipratipadyate ।।

alayaṃs tu bhiṣag-bruvaḥ alpayaṃs tu bhiṣag dhruvam
tato alpam alpa-vīryaṃ vā guru-vyādhau prayojitam ।
udīrayet-tarāṃ rogān saṃśodhanam a-yogataḥ ।।

śodhanaṃ tv ati-yogena viparītaṃ viparyaye ।
kṣiṇuyān na malān eva kevalaṃ vapur asyati ।।

evalaṃ vapur apy ati
ato abhiyuktaḥ satataṃ sarvam ālocya sarva-thā ।
tathā yuñjīta bhaiṣajyam ārogyāya yathā dhruvam ।।

ārogyāya yathā bhavet
vakṣyante ataḥ paraṃ doṣā vṛddhi-kṣaya-vibhedataḥ ।
pṛthak trīn viddhi saṃsargas tri-dhā tatra tu tān nava ।।

ṛthak trīn viddhi saṃsargaṃ
trīn eva samayā vṛddhyā ṣaḍ ekasyātiśāyane ।
trayo-daśa samasteṣu ṣaḍ dvy-ekātiśayena tu ।।

ṣaḍ dvy-ekātiśayena ca
ekaṃ tulyādhikaiḥ ṣaṭ ca tāratamya-vikalpanāt ।
pañca-viṃśatim ity evaṃ vṛddhaiḥ kṣīṇaiś ca tāvataḥ ।।

añca-viṃśatir ity evaṃ
ekaika-vṛddhi-sama-tā-kṣayaiḥ ṣaṭ te punaś ca ṣaṭ ।
eka-kṣaya-dvandva-vṛddhyā sa-viparyayayāpi te ।।
bhedā dvi-ṣaṣṭir nirdiṣṭās tri-ṣaṣṭiḥ svāsthya-kāraṇam ।।saṃsargād rasa-rudhirādibhis tathaiṣāṃ ।।
aṃsargād rasa-rudhirādibhis tathaitān doṣāṃs tu kṣaya-sama-tā-vivṛddhi-bhedaiḥ ।।

oṣāṇāṃ kṣaya-sama-tā-vivṛddhi-bhedaiḥ ānantyaṃ tara-tama-yogataś ca yātān ।।
jānīyād avahita-mānaso yathā-svam ।।
sūtrasthāna
vātasyopakramaḥ snehaḥ svedaḥ saṃśodhanaṃ mṛdu ।
svādv-amla-lavaṇoṣṇāni bhojyāny abhyaṅga-mardanam ।।

veṣṭanaṃ trāsanaṃ seko madyaṃ paiṣṭika-gauḍikam ।
snigdhoṣṇā vastayo vasti-niyamaḥ sukha-śīla-tā ।।

dīpanaiḥ pācanaiḥ snigdhāḥ snehāś cāneka-yonayaḥ ।
viśeṣān medya-piśita-rasa-tailānuvāsanam ।।

pittasya sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ svādu-śītair virecanam ।
svādu-tikta-kaṣāyāṇi bhojanāny auṣadhāni ca ।।

su-gandhi-śīta-hṛdyānāṃ gandhānām upasevanam ।
kaṇṭhe-guṇānāṃ hārāṇāṃ maṇīnām urasā dhṛtiḥ ।।

karpūra-candanośīrair anulepaḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe ।
pradoṣaś candramāḥ saudhaṃ hāri gītaṃ himo anilaḥ ।।

a-yantraṇa-sukhaṃ mitraṃ putraḥ saṃdigdha-mugdha-vāk ।
chandānuvartino dārāḥ priyāḥ śīla-vibhūṣitāḥ ।।

-yantraṇa-mukhaṃ mitraṃ
śītāmbu-dhārā-garbhāṇi gṛhāṇy udyāna-dīrghikāḥ ।
su-tīrtha-vipula-svaccha-salilāśaya-saikate ।।

sāmbho-ja-jala-tīrānte kāyamāne drumākule ।
saumyā bhāvāḥ payaḥ sarpir virekaś ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

āyamānaṃ drumākule
śleṣmaṇo vidhinā yuktaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ vamana-recanam ।
annaṃ rūkṣālpa-tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ kaṭu-tikta-kaṣāyakam ।।

dīrgha-kāla-sthitaṃ madyaṃ rati-prītiḥ prajāgaraḥ ।
aneka-rūpo vyāyāmaś cintā rūkṣaṃ vimardanam ।।

viśeṣād vamanaṃ yūṣaḥ kṣaudraṃ medo-ghnam auṣadham ।
dhūmopavāsa-gaṇḍūṣā niḥ-sukha-tvaṃ sukhāya ca ।।

upakramaḥ pṛthag doṣān yo ayam uddiśya kīrtitaḥ ।
saṃsarga-saṃnipāteṣu taṃ yathā-svaṃ vikalpayet ।।

aṃ yathā-svaṃ prakalpayet
graiṣmaḥ prāyo marut-pitte vāsantaḥ kapha-mārute ।
maruto yoga-vāhi-tvāt kapha-pitte tu śāradaḥ ।।

caya eva jayed doṣaṃ kupitaṃ tv a-virodhayan ।
sarva-kope balīyāṃsaṃ śeṣa-doṣā-virodhataḥ ।।

prayogaḥ śamayed vyādhim ekaṃ yo anyam udīrayet ।
nāsau viśuddhaḥ śuddhas tu śamayed yo na kopayet ।।

rayogaḥ śamayed vyādhiṃ o anyam anyam udīrayet
vyāyāmād ūṣmaṇas taikṣṇyād a-hitācaraṇād api ।
koṣṭhāc chākhāsthi-marmāṇi druta-tvān mārutasya ca ।।

doṣā yānti tathā tebhyaḥ sroto-mukha-viśodhanāt ।
vṛddhyābhiṣyandanāt pākāt koṣṭhaṃ vāyoś ca nigrahāt ।।

tatra-sthāś ca vilamberan bhūyo hetu-pratīkṣiṇaḥ ।
te kālādi-balaṃ labdhvā kupyanty anyāśrayeṣv api ।।

tatrānya-sthāna-saṃstheṣu tadīyām a-baleṣu tu ।
kuryāc cikitsāṃ svām eva balenānyābhibhāviṣu ।।

āgantuṃ śamayed doṣaṃ sthāninaṃ pratikṛtya vā ।
prāyas tiryag-gatā doṣāḥ kleśayanty āturāṃś ciram ।।
sādhāraṇaṃ vā kurvīta kriyām ubhaya-yoginīm ।।
kuryān na teṣu tvarayā dehāgni-bala-vit kriyām ।
śamayet tān prayogeṇa sukhaṃ vā koṣṭham ānayet ।।

jñātvā koṣṭha-prapannāṃś ca yathāsannaṃ vinirharet ।
sroto-rodha-bala-bhraṃśa-gauravānila-mūḍha-tāḥ ।।

-gauravānila-mūḍha-tā
ālasyā-pakti-niṣṭhīva-mala-saṅgā-ruci-klamāḥ ।
liṅgaṃ malānāṃ sāmānāṃ nir-āmāṇāṃ viparyayaḥ ।।

viṇ-mūtra-nakha-danta-tvak-cakṣuṣāṃ pīta-tā bhavet ।
rakta-tvam atha kṛṣṇa-tvaṃ pṛṣṭhāsthi-kaṭi-saṃdhi-ruk ।।

ṛṣṭhāsthi-kaṭi-saṃdhiṣu
śiro-ruk jāyate tīvrā nidrā vi-rasa-tā mukhe ।
kva-cic ca śvayathur gātre jvarātīsāra-harṣaṇam ।।

ūṣmaṇo alpa-bala-tvena dhātum ādyam a-pācitam ।
duṣṭam āmāśaya-gataṃ rasam āmaṃ pracakṣate ।।

anye doṣebhya evāti-duṣṭebhyo anyo-'nya-mūrchanāt ।
kodravebhyo viṣasyeva vadanty āmasya saṃbhavam ।।

āmena tena saṃpṛktā doṣā dūṣyāś ca dūṣitāḥ ।
sāmā ity upadiśyante ye ca rogās tad-udbhavāḥ ।।

vāyuḥ sāmo vibandhāgni-sāda-stambhāntra-kūjanaiḥ ।
vedanā-śopha-nistodaiḥ krama-śo aṅgāni pīḍayan ।।

vicared yuga-pac cāpi gṛhṇāti kupito bhṛśam ।
snehādyair vṛddhim āyāti sūrya-meghodaye niśi ।।

nir-āmo viśado rūkṣo nir-vibandho alpa-vedanaḥ ।
viparīta-guṇaiḥ śāntiṃ snigdhair yāti viśeṣataḥ ।।

dur-gandhi haritaṃ śyāvaṃ pittam amlaṃ ghanaṃ guru ।
amlīkā-kaṇṭha-hṛd-dāha-karaṃ sāmaṃ vinirdiśet ।।

ā-tāmra-pītam aty-uṣṇaṃ rase kaṭukam a-sthiram ।
pakvaṃ vi-gandhi vijñeyaṃ ruci-pakti-bala-pradam ।।

uci-vahni-bala-pradam
āvilas tantulaḥ styānaḥ kaṇṭha-deśe avatiṣṭhate ।
sāmo balāso dur-gandhiḥ kṣud-udgāra-vighāta-kṛt ।।

phena-vān piṇḍitaḥ pāṇdur niḥ-sāro a-gandha eva ca ।
pakvaḥ sa eva vijñeyaś cheda-vān vaktra-śuddhi-daḥ ।।

sarva-deha-pravisṛtān sāmān doṣān na nirharet ।
līnān dhātuṣv an-utkliṣṭān phalād āmād rasān iva ।।

āśrayasya hi nāśāya te syur dur-nirhara-tvataḥ ।
pācanair dīpanaiḥ snehais tān svedaiś ca pariṣkṛtān ।।

śodhayec chodhanaiḥ kāle yathāsannaṃ yathā-balam ।
hanty āśu yuktaṃ vaktreṇa dravyam āmāśayān malān ।।

ghrāṇena cordhva-jatrūtthān pakvādhānād gudena ca ।
utkliṣṭān adha ūrdhvaṃ vā na cāmān vahataḥ svayam ।।

dhārayed auṣadhair doṣān vidhṛtās te hi roga-dāḥ ।
pravṛttān prāg ato doṣān upekṣeta hitāśinaḥ ।।

vibaddhān pācanais tais taiḥ pācayen nirhareta vā ।
śrāvaṇe kārttike caitre māsi sādhāraṇe kramāt ।।

ācayen nirharet tathā
prāvṛṭ-śarad-vasanteṣu māseṣv eteṣu śodhayet ।
sādhāraṇeṣu vidhinā tri-māsāntaritān malān ।।

grīṣma-varṣā-hima-citān vāyv-ādīn āśu nirharet ।
aty-uṣṇa-varṣa-śītā hi grīṣma-varṣā-himāgamāḥ ।।

saṃdhau sādhāraṇe teṣāṃ duṣṭān doṣān viśodhayet ।
svastha-vṛttam abhipretya vyādhau vyādhi-vaśena tu ।।

trayaḥ sādhāraṇās teṣām antare prāvṛṣādayaḥ ।
prāvṛṭ śuci-nabhau teṣu śarad ūrja-sahau smṛtau ।।

tapasyo madhu-māsaś ca vasantaḥ śodhanaṃ prati ।
etān ṛtūn vikalpyaivaṃ dadyāt saṃśodhanaṃ bhiṣak ।।

kṛtvā śītoṣṇa-vṛṣṭīnāṃ pratīkāraṃ yathā-yatham ।
prayojayet kriyāṃ prāptāṃ kriyā-kālaṃ na hāpayet ।।

yuñjyād an-annam annādau madhye ante kavaḍāntare ।
grāse grāse muhuḥ sānnaṃ sāmudgaṃ niśi cauṣadham ।।

kaphodreke gade an-annaṃ balino roga-rogiṇoḥ ।
annādau vi-guṇe apāne samāne madhya iṣyate ।।

vyāne ante prātar-āśasya sāyam-āśasya tūttare ।
grāsa-grāsāntayoḥ prāṇe praduṣṭe mātariśvani ।।

muhur muhur viṣa-cchardi-hidhmā-tṛṭ-śvāsa-kāsiṣu ।
yojyaṃ sa-bhojyaṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ bhojyaiś citrair a-rocake ।।

kampākṣepaka-hidhmāsu sāmudgaṃ laghu-bhojinām ।
ūrdhva-jatru-vikāreṣu svapna-kāle praśasyate ।।

sūtrasthāna
upakramyasya hi dvi-tvād dvi-dhaivopakramo mataḥ ।
ekaḥ saṃtarpaṇas tatra dvitīyaś cāpatarpaṇaḥ ।।

bṛṃhaṇo laṅghanaś ceti tat-paryāyāv udāhṛtau ।
bṛṃhaṇaṃ yad bṛhat-tvāya laṅghanaṃ lāghavāya yat ।।

dehasya bhavataḥ prāyo bhaumāpam itarac ca te ।
snehanaṃ rūkṣaṇaṃ karma svedanaṃ stambhanaṃ ca yat ।।

bhūtānāṃ tad api dvaidhyād dvitayaṃ nātivartate ।
śodhanaṃ śamanaṃ ceti dvi-dhā tatrāpi laṅghanam ।।

yad īrayed bahir doṣān pañca-dhā śodhanaṃ ca tat ।
nirūho vamanaṃ kāya-śiro-reko asra-visrutiḥ ।।

na śodhayati yad doṣān samān nodīrayaty api ।
samī-karoti viṣamān śamanaṃ tac ca sapta-dhā ।।

pācanaṃ dīpanaṃ kṣut-tṛḍ-vyāyāmātapa-mārutāḥ ।
bṛṃhaṇaṃ śamanaṃ tv eva vāyoḥ pittānilasya ca ।।

bṛṃhayed vyādhi-bhaiṣajya-madya-strī-śoka-karśitān ।
bhārādhvoraḥ-kṣata-kṣīṇa-rūkṣa-dur-bala-vātalān ।।

garbhiṇī-sūtikā-bāla-vṛddhān grīṣme aparān api ।
māṃsa-kṣīra-sitā-sarpir-madhura-snigdha-vastibhiḥ ।।

svapna-śayyā-sukhābhyaṅga-snāna-nirvṛti-harṣaṇaiḥ ।
mehāma-doṣāti-snigdha-jvaroru-stambha-kuṣṭhinaḥ ।।

visarpa-vidradhi-plīha-śiraḥ-kaṇṭhākṣi-rogiṇaḥ ।
sthūlāṃś ca laṅghayen nityaṃ śiśire tv aparān api ।।

tatra saṃśodhanaiḥ sthaulya-bala-pitta-kaphādhikān ।
āma-doṣa-jvara-cchardir-atīsāra-hṛd-āmayaiḥ ।।

vibandha-gauravodgāra-hṛl-lāsādibhir āturān ।
madhya-sthaulyādikān prāyaḥ pūrvaṃ pācana-dīpanaiḥ ।।

ebhir evāmayair ārtān hīna-sthaulya-balādhikān ।
kṣut-tṛṣṇā-nigrahair doṣais tv ārtān madhya-balair dṛḍhān ।।

ṣut-tṛṣṇā-nigrahair doṣair ṣut-tṛṣṇā-nigrahair doṣaiś 
ārtān madhya-balair dṛḍhān
samīraṇātapāyāsaiḥ kim utālpa-balair narān ।
na bṛṃhayel laṅghanīyān bṛṃhyāṃs tu mṛdu laṅghayet ।।

yuktyā vā deśa-kālādi-balatas tān upācaret ।
bṛṃhite syād balaṃ puṣṭis tat-sādhyāmaya-saṃkṣayaḥ ।।

vi-malendriya-tā sargo malānāṃ lāghavaṃ ruciḥ ।
kṣut-tṛṭ-sahodayaḥ śuddha-hṛdayodgāra-kaṇṭha-tā ।।

vyādhi-mārdavam utsāhas tandrā-nāśaś ca laṅghite ।
an-apekṣita-mātrādi-sevite kurutas tu te ।।

ati-sthaulyāti-kārśyādīn vakṣyante te ca sauṣadhāḥ ।
rūpaṃ tair eva ca jñeyam ati-bṛṃhita-laṅghite ।।

ūpaṃ tair eva vijñeyam
ati-sthaulyāpacī-meha-jvarodara-bhagandarān ।
kāsa-saṃnyāsa-kṛcchrāma-kuṣṭhādīn ati-dāruṇān ।।

tatra medo-'nila-śleṣma-nāśanaṃ sarvam iṣyate ।
kulattha-jūrṇa-śyāmāka-yava-mudga-madhūdakam ।।

mastu-daṇḍāhatāriṣṭa-cintā-śodhana-jāgaram ।
madhunā tri-phalāṃ lihyād guḍūcīm abhayāṃ ghanam ।।

rasāñjanasya mahataḥ pañca-mūlasya gugguloḥ ।
śilā-jatu-prayogaś ca sāgnimantha-raso hitaḥ ।।

śilāhvasya prayogaś ca
viḍaṅgaṃ nāgaraṃ kṣāraḥ kāla-loha-rajo madhu ।
yavāmalaka-cūrṇaṃ ca yogo ati-sthaulya-doṣa-jit ।।

vyoṣa-kaṭvī-varā-śigru-viḍaṅgātiviṣā-sthirāḥ ।
hiṅgu-sauvarcalājājī-yavānī-dhānya-citrakāḥ ।।

niśe bṛhatyau hapuṣā pāṭhā mūlaṃ ca kembukāt ।
eṣāṃ cūrṇaṃ madhu ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ ca sadṛśāṃśakam ।।

ailaṃ ca sadṛśāṃśikam
saktubhiḥ ṣo-ḍaśa-guṇair yuktaṃ pītaṃ nihanti tat ।
ati-sthaulyādikān sarvān rogān anyāṃś ca tad-vidhān ।।

hṛd-roga-kāmalā-śvitra-śvāsa-kāsa-gala-grahān ।
buddhi-medhā-smṛti-karaṃ saṃnasyāgneś ca dīpanam ।।

ati-kārśyaṃ bhramaḥ kāsas tṛṣṇādhikyam a-rocakaḥ ।
snehāgni-nidrā-dṛk-śrotra-śukraujaḥ-kṣut-svara-kṣayaḥ ।।

ti-kārśyaṃ bhramaḥ śvāsa- -tṛṣṇādhikyam a-rocakaḥ
vasti-hṛn-mūrdha-jaṅghoru-trika-pārśva-rujā jvaraḥ ।
pralāpordhvānila-glāni-cchardi-parvāsthi-bhedanam ।।

-cchardiḥ-parvāsthi-bhedanam
varco-mūtra-grahādyāś ca jāyante ati-vilaṅghanāt ।
kārśyam eva varaṃ sthaulyān na hi sthūlasya bheṣajam ।।

iṇ-mūtrādi-grahādyāś ca a hi sthaulyasya bheṣajam
bṛṃhaṇaṃ laṅghanaṃ vālam ati-medo-'gni-vāta-jit ।
madhura-snigdha-sauhityair yat saukhyena ca naśyati ।।

ṛṃhaṇaṃ laṅghanaṃ nālam adhura-sneha-sauhityair 
at saukhyena vinaśyati
kraśimā sthavimāty-anta-viparīta-niṣevaṇaiḥ ।
yojayed bṛṃhaṇaṃ tatra sarvaṃ pānānna-bheṣajam ।।

a-cintayā harṣaṇena dhruvaṃ saṃtarpaṇena ca ।
svapna-prasaṅgāc ca kṛśo varāha iva puṣyati ।।

-cintayā praharṣeṇa vapna-prasaṅgāc ca naro
na hi māṃsa-samaṃ kiñ-cid anyad deha-bṛhat-tva-kṛt ।
māṃsāda-māṃsaṃ māṃsena saṃbhṛta-tvād viśeṣataḥ ।।

aṃbhṛta-tvād viśiṣyate aṃbhṛta-tvād bṛhat-tva-kṛt
guru cā-tarpaṇaṃ sthūle viparītaṃ hitaṃ kṛśe ।
yava-godhūmam ubhayos tad-yogyāhita-kalpanam ।।

ad-yogya-hita-kalpanam ato grāhita-kalpanam
doṣa-gatyātiricyante grāhi-bhedy-ādi-bhedataḥ ।
upakramā na te dvi-tvād bhinnā api gadā iva ।।

pakramā na tu dvi-tvād

sūtrasthāna
madana-madhuka-lambā-nimba-bimbī-viśālā-trapusa-kuṭaja-mūrvā-devadālī-kṛmighnam ।
vidula-dahana-citrāḥ kośavatyau karañjaḥ kaṇa-lavaṇa-vacailā-sarṣapāś chardanāni ।। 

।।

nikumbha-kumbha-tri-phalā-gavākṣī-snuk-śaṅkhinī-nīlini-tilvakāni ।
śamyāka-kampillaka-hemadugdhā dugdhaṃ ca mūtraṃ ca virecanāni ।।

madana-kuṭaja-kuṣṭha-devadālī-madhuka-vacā-daśa-mūla-dāru-rāsnāḥ ।
yava-miśi-kṛtavedhanaṃ kulatthā madhu lavaṇaṃ trivṛtā nirūhaṇāni ।।

ava-miśi-kṛtavedhanaṃ kulattho
vellāpāmārga-vyoṣa-dārvī-surālā bījaṃ śairīṣaṃ bārhataṃ śaigravaṃ ca ।
sāro mādhūkaḥ saindhavaṃ tārkṣya-śailaṃ truṭyau pṛthvīkā śodhayanty uttamāṅgam ।। 

।।

bhadradāru nataṃ kuṣṭhaṃ daśa-mūlaṃ balā-dvayam ।
vāyuṃ vīratarādiś ca vidāry-ādiś ca nāśayet ।।

aśa-mūlaṃ balā-trayam idāry-ādiś ca śodhayet
dūrvānantā nimba-vāsātmaguptā gundrābhīruḥ śītapākī priyaṅguḥ ।
nyagrodhādiḥ padmakādiḥ sthire dve padmaṃ vanyaṃ śārivādiś ca pittam ।।

āragvadhādir arkādir muṣkakādyo asanādikaḥ ।
surasādiḥ sa-mustādir vatsakādir balāsa-jit ।।

jīvantī-kākolyau mede dve mudga-māṣaparṇyau ca ।
ṛṣabhaka-jīvaka-madhukaṃ ceti gaṇo jīvanīyākhyaḥ ।।

vidāri-pañcāṅgula-vṛścikālī-vṛścīva-devāhvaya-śūrpaparṇyaḥ ।
kaṇḍūkarī jīvana-hrasva-saṃjñe dve pañcake gopasutā tripādī ।।

-vṛścīva-devā-dvaya-śūrpaparṇyaḥ aṇḍūkarī gopasutā tripādī
vidāry-ādir ayaṃ hṛdyo bṛṃhaṇo vāta-pitta-hā ।
śoṣa-gulmāṅga-mardordhva-śvāsa-kāsa-haro gaṇaḥ ।।

śoṣa-gulmāṅga-sādordhva-
śārivośīra-kāśmarya-madhūka-śiśira-dvayam ।
yaṣṭī parūṣakaṃ hanti dāha-pittāsra-tṛḍ-jvarān ।।

padmaka-puṇḍrau vṛddhi-tugarddhyaḥ śṛṅgy amṛtā daśa jīvana-saṃjñāḥ ।
stanya-karā ghnantīraṇa-pittaṃ prīṇana-jīvana-bṛṃhaṇa-vṛṣyāḥ ।।

parūṣakaṃ varā drākṣā kaṭphalaṃ katakāt phalam ।
rājāhvaṃ dāḍimaṃ śākaṃ tṛṇ-mūtrāmaya-vāta-jit ।।

añjanaṃ phalinī māṃsī padmotpala-rasāñjanam ।
sailā-madhuka-nāgāhvaṃ viṣāntar-dāha-pitta-nut ।।

iṣāntar-dāha-pitta-jit iṣāntar-dāha-pitta-hṛt
paṭola-kaṭu-rohiṇī-candanaṃ madhusrava-guḍūci-pāṭhānvitam ।
nihanti kapha-pitta-kuṣṭha-jvarān viṣaṃ vamim a-rocakaṃ kāmalām ।।

guḍūcī-padmakāriṣṭa-dhānakā-rakta-candanam ।
pitta-śleṣma-jvara-cchardi-dāha-tṛṣṇā-ghnam agni-kṛt ।।

-dhānyakā-rakta-candanam -dhānyakaṃ rakta-candanam 
-dhanikā-rakta-candanam
āragvadhendrayava-pāṭali-kākatiktā-nimbāmṛtā-madhurasā-sruva-vṛkṣa-pāṭhāḥ ।
bhūnimba-sairyaka-paṭola-karañja-yugma-saptacchadāgni-suṣavī-phala-bāṇa-ghoṇṭāḥ ।।

।।

āragvadhādir jayati cchardi-kuṣṭha-viṣa-jvarān ।
kaphaṃ kaṇḍūṃ pramehaṃ ca duṣṭa-vraṇa-viśodhanaḥ ।।

edodara-viśodhanaḥ
asana-tiniśa-bhūrja-śvetavāha-prakīryāḥ khadira-kadara-bhaṇḍī-śiṃśipā-meṣaśṛṅgyaḥ ।
tri-hima-tala-palāśā joṅgakaḥ śāka-śālau kramuka-dhava-kaliṅga-cchāgakarṇāśvakarṇāḥ ।।

।।

asanādir vijayate śvitra-kuṣṭha-kapha-krimīn ।
pāṇḍu-rogaṃ pramehaṃ ca medo-doṣa-nibarhaṇaḥ ।।

śvitra-kuṣṭha-vami-krimīn
varuṇa-sairyaka-yugma-śatāvarī-dahana-moraṭa-bilva-viṣāṇikāḥ ।
dvi-bṛhatī-dvi-karañja-jayā-dvayaṃ bahalapallava-darbha-rujākarāḥ ।।

araṇa-sairyaka-yugma-śatāvarī-
varuṇādiḥ kaphaṃ medo mandāgni-tvaṃ niyacchati ।
āḍhya-vātaṃ śiraḥ-śūlaṃ gulmaṃ cāntaḥ sa-vidradhim ।।

araṇādiḥ kaphaṃ medo dho-vātaṃ śiraḥ-śūlaṃ
ūṣakas tutthakaṃ hiṅgu kāsīsa-dvaya-saindhavam ।
sa-śilā-jatu kṛcchrāśma-gulma-medaḥ-kaphāpaham ।।

-gulma-meha-kaphāpaham
vellantarāraṇika-būka-vṛṣāśmabheda-gokaṇṭaketkaṭa-sahācara-bāṇa-kāśāḥ ।
vṛkṣādanī-nala-kuśa-dvaya-guṇṭha-gundrā-bhallūka-moraṭa-kuraṇṭa-karambha-pārthāḥ ।।

।।

-gokaṇṭakotkaṭa-sahācara-bāṇa-kāśāḥ ṛkṣādanī-nala-kuśa-dvaya-guntha-gundrā- ṛkṣādanī-nala-kuśa-dvaya-guñcha-gundrā- 
vṛkṣādanī-nala-kuśa-dvaya-guccha-gundrā-
vargo vīratarādyo ayaṃ hanti vāta-kṛtān gadān ।
aśmarī-śarkarā-mūtra-kṛcchrāghāta-rujā-haraḥ ।।

-kṛcchrāghāta-rujāpahaḥ
lodhra-śābaraka-lodhra-palāśā jiṅginī-sarala-kaṭphala-yuktāḥ ।
kutsitāmba-kadalī-gataśokāḥ sailavālu-paripelava-mocāḥ ।।

odhra-śābara-kadamba-palāśā hiñjhiṇī-sarala-kaṭphala-yuktāḥ
eṣa lodhrādiko nāma medaḥ-kapha-haro gaṇaḥ ।
yoni-doṣa-haraḥ stambhī varṇyo viṣa-vināśanaḥ ।।

arkālarkau nāgadantī viśalyā bhārgī rāsnā vṛścikālī prakīryā ।
pratyakpuṣpī pītatailodakīryā śvetā-yugmaṃ tāpasānāṃ ca vṛkṣaḥ ।।

ayam arkādiko vargaḥ kapha-medo-viṣāpahaḥ ।
kṛmi-kuṣṭha-praśamano viśeṣād vraṇa-śodhanaḥ ।।

yam arkādiko nāma
surasa-yuga-phaṇijjaṃ kālamālā viḍaṅgaṃ kharabusa-vṛṣakarṇī-kaṭphalaṃ kāsamardaḥ ।
kṣavaka-sarasi-bhārgī-kārmukāḥ kākamācī kulahala-viṣamuṣṭī bhūstṛṇo bhūtakeśī ।। 

।।

harabuka-vṛṣakarṇī-kaṭphalāḥ kāsamardaḥ harabusa-vṛṣakarṇī-kaṭphalāḥ kāsamardaḥ c kharamukha-vṛṣakarṇī-kaṭphalaṃ kāsamardaḥ ṣavaka-surasi-bhārgī-kārmukāḥ kākamācī ṣavaka-surasi-bhārgī-kāmukāḥ kākamācī ṣavaka-sarasi-bhārgī-kāmukāḥ kākamācī 
ṣavaka-svarasi-bhārgī-kārmukāḥ kākamācī
surasādir gaṇaḥ śleṣma-medaḥ-kṛmi-niṣūdanaḥ ।
pratiśyāyā-ruci-śvāsa-kāsa-ghno vraṇa-śodhanaḥ ।।

muṣkaka-snug-varā-dvīpi-palāśa-dhava-śiṃśipāḥ ।
gulma-mehāśmarī-pāṇḍu-medo-'rśaḥ-kapha-śukra-jit ।।

-palāśa-dhava-śiṃśipam
vatsaka-mūrvā-bhārgī-kaṭukā marīcaṃ ghuṇapriyā ca gaṇḍīram ।
elā pāṭhājājī kaṭvaṅga-phalājamoda-siddhārtha-vacāḥ ।।

jīraka-hiṅgu-viḍaṅgaṃ paśugandhā pañca-kolakaṃ hanti ।
cala-kapha-medaḥ-pīnasa-gulma-jvara-śūla-dur-nāmnaḥ ।।

aśugandhā pañca-kolakaṃ ghnanti
vacā-jalada-devāhva-nāgarātiviṣābhayāḥ ।
haridrā-dvaya-yaṣṭy-āhva-kalaśī-kuṭajodbhavāḥ ।।

vacā-haridrādi-gaṇāv āmātīsāra-nāśanau ।
medaḥ-kaphāḍhya-pavana-stanya-doṣa-nibarhaṇau ।।

āmātīsāra-pācanau
priyaṅgu-puṣpāñjana-yugma-padmāḥ padmād rajo yojanavally anantā ।
mānadrumo moca-rasaḥ samaṅgā punnāga-śītaṃ madanīya-hetuḥ ।।

āradrumo moca-rasaḥ samaṅgā unnāma-śītaṃ 
madanīya-hetuḥ
ambaṣṭhā madhukaṃ namaskarī nandīvṛkṣa-palāśa-kacchurāḥ ।
lodhraṃ dhātaki-bilva-peśike kaṭvaṅgaḥ kamalodbhavaṃ rajaḥ ।।

gaṇau priyaṅgv-ambaṣṭhādī pakvātīsāra-nāśanau ।
saṃdhānīyau hitau pitte vraṇānām api ropaṇau ।।

mustā-vacāgni-dvi-niśā-dvi-tiktā-bhallāta-pāṭhā-tri-phalā-viṣākhyāḥ ।
kuṣṭhaṃ truṭī haimavatī ca yoni-stanyāmaya-ghnā mala-pācanāś ca ।।

nyagrodha-pippala-sadāphala-lodhra-yugmaṃ jambū-dvayārjuna-kapītana-somavalkāḥ ।
plakṣāmra-vañjula-piyāla-palāśa-nandī-kolī-kadamba-viralā-madhukaṃ madhūkam ।। 

।।

yagrodha-pippala-sadāphala-lodhra-yugma- 
-jambū-dvayārjuna-kapītana-somavalkāḥ
nyagrodhādir gaṇo vraṇyaḥ saṃgrāhī bhagna-sādhanaḥ ।
medaḥ-pittāsra-tṛḍ-dāha-yoni-roga-nibarhaṇaḥ ।।

yagrodhādir gaṇo varṇyaḥ -yoni-doṣa-nibarhaṇaḥ elā-yugma-turuṣka-kuṣṭha-phalinī-māṃsī-jala-dhyāmakaṃ ।।
spṛkkā-coraka-coca-pattra-tagara-sthauṇeya-jātī-rasāḥ ।।
-spṛkkā-coraka-coca-pattra-tagara-sthauṇeya-jātī-rasāḥ śuktir vyāghranakho amarāhvam aguruḥ śrīvāsakaḥ kuṅkumaṃ ।।

śuktir vyāghranakho amarāhvam aguruḥ śrīvāsakaṃ kuṅkumaṃ
śukti-vyāghranakhau surāhvam aguruḥ śrīveṣṭakaḥ kuṅkumaṃ
caṇḍā-guggulu-deva-dhūpa-khapurāḥ punnāga-nāgāhvayam ।।

elādiko vāta-kaphau viṣaṃ ca viniyacchati ।
varṇa-prasādanaḥ kaṇḍū-piṭikā-koṭha-nāśanaḥ ।।

arṇyaḥ prasādanaḥ kaṇḍū- śyāmā-dantī-dravantī-kramuka-kuṭaraṇā-śaṅkhinī-carma-sāhvā- ।।

śyāmā-dantī-dravantī-kramuka-kuṭaraṇī-śaṅkhinī-carma-sāhvā- -svarṇakṣīrī-gavākṣī-śikhari-rajanaka-cchinnarohā-karañjāḥ ।।
bastāntrī vyādhighāto bahala-bahu-rasas tīkṣṇavṛkṣāt phalāni ।।
astāntrī vyādhighāto bahula-bahu-rasas tīkṣṇavṛkṣāt phalāni śyāmādyo hanti gulmaṃ viṣama-ruci-kaphau hṛd-rujaṃ mūtra-kṛcchram ।।

trayas-triṃśad iti proktā vargās teṣu tv a-lābhataḥ ।
yuñjyāt tad-vidham anyac ca dravyaṃ jahyād a-yaugikam ।।

ete vargā doṣa-dūṣyādy apekṣya kalka-kvātha-sneha-lehādi-yuktāḥ ।
pāne nasye anvāsane antar bahir vā lepābhyaṅgair ghnanti rogān su-kṛcchrān ।।

te vargā doṣa-dūṣyādy avekṣya ekālepair ghnanti rogān su-kṛcchrān vedābhyaṅgair ghnanti rogān su-kṛcchrān

sūtrasthāna
guru-śīta-sara-snigdha-manda-sūkṣma-mṛdu-dravam ।
auṣadhaṃ snehanaṃ prāyo viparītaṃ virūkṣaṇam ।।

sarpir majjā vasā tailaṃ sneheṣu pravaraṃ matam ।
tatrāpi cottamaṃ sarpiḥ saṃskārasyānuvartanāt ।।

mādhuryād a-vidāhi-tvāj janmādy eva ca śīlanāt ।
pitta-ghnās te yathā-pūrvam itara-ghnā yathottaram ।।

ghṛtāt tailaṃ guru vasā tailān majjā tato api ca ।
dvābhyāṃ tribhiś caturbhis tair yamakas tri-vṛto mahān ।।

svedya-saṃśodhya-madya-strī-vyāyāmāsakta-cintakāḥ ।
vṛddha-bālā-bala-kṛśā rūkṣāḥ kṣīṇāsra-retasaḥ ।।

vātārta-syanda-timira-dāruṇa-pratibodhinaḥ ।
snehyā na tv ati-mandāgni-tīkṣṇāgni-sthūla-dur-balāḥ ।।

ūru-stambhātisārāma-gala-roga-garodaraiḥ ।
mūrchā-chardy-a-ruci-śleṣma-tṛṣṇā-madyaiś ca pīḍitāḥ ।।

apaprasūtā yukte ca nasye vastau virecane ।
tatra dhī-smṛti-medhādi-kāṅkṣiṇāṃ śasyate ghṛtam ।।

atra dhī-smṛti-medhāgni-
granthi-nāḍī-kṛmi-śleṣma-medo-māruta-rogiṣu ।
tailaṃ lāghava-dārḍhyārthi-krūra-koṣṭheṣu dehiṣu ।।

vātātapādhva-bhāra-strī-vyāyāma-kṣīṇa-dhātuṣu ।
rūkṣa-kleśa-kṣamāty-agni-vātāvṛta-patheṣu ca ।।

śeṣau vasā tu saṃdhy-asthi-marma-koṣṭha-rujāsu ca ।
tathā dagdhāhata-bhraṣṭa-yoni-karṇa-śiro-ruji ।।

tailaṃ prāvṛṣi varṣānte sarpir anyau tu mādhave ।
ṛtau sādhāraṇe snehaḥ śasto ahni vi-male ravau ।।

tailaṃ tvarāyāṃ śīte api gharme api ca ghṛtaṃ niśi ।
niśy eva pitte pavane saṃsarge pitta-vaty api ।।

niśy anya-thā vāta-kaphād rogāḥ syuḥ pittato divā ।
yuktyāvacārayet snehaṃ bhakṣyādy-annena vastibhiḥ ।।

nasyābhyañjana-gaṇḍūṣa-mūrdha-karṇākṣi-tarpaṇaiḥ ।
rasa-bhedaikaka-tvābhyāṃ catuḥ-ṣaṣṭir vicāraṇāḥ ।।

snehasyānyābhibhūta-tvād alpa-tvāc ca kramāt smṛtāḥ ।
yathokta-hetv-a-bhāvāc ca nāccha-peyo vicāraṇā ।।

nehasyānnābhibhūta-tvād ācchaḥ peyo vicāraṇā
snehasya kalpaḥ sa śreṣṭhaḥ sneha-karmāśu-sādhanāt ।
dvābhyāṃ caturbhir aṣṭābhir yāmair jīryanti yāḥ kramāt ।।

hrasva-madhyottamā mātrās tās tābhyaś ca hrasīyasīm ।
kalpayed vīkṣya doṣādīn prāg eva tu hrasīyasīm ।।

hyastane jīrṇa evānne sneho acchaḥ śuddhaye bahuḥ ।
śamanaḥ kṣud-vato an-anno madhya-mātraś ca śasyate ।।

bṛṃhaṇo rasa-madyādyaiḥ sa-bhakto alpo hitaḥ sa ca ।
bāla-vṛddha-pipāsārta-sneha-dviṇ-madya-śīliṣu ।।

a-bhakto alpo hitaś ca saḥ
strī-sneha-nitya-mandāgni-sukhita-kleśa-bhīruṣu ।
mṛdu-koṣṭhālpa-doṣeṣu kāle coṣṇe kṛśeṣu ca ।।

prāṅ-madhyottara-bhakto asāv adho-madhyordhva-deha-jān ।
vyādhīñ jayed balaṃ kuryād aṅgānāṃ ca yathā-kramam ।।

vāry uṣṇam acche anupibet snehe tat sukha-paktaye ।
āsyopalepa-śuddhyai ca taubarāruṣkare na tu ।।

mūrchā dāho a-ratis tṛṣṇā jṛmbhā moha-bhrama-klamāḥ ।
bhavanti jīryati snehe jīrṇaḥ syāt taiḥ śamaṃ gataiḥ ।।

jīrṇā-jīrṇa-viśaṅkāyāṃ punar uṣṇodakaṃ pibet ।
tenodgāra-viśuddhiḥ syāt tataś ca laghu-tā ruciḥ ।।

bhojyo annaṃ mātrayā pāsyan śvaḥ piban pīta-vān api ।
dravoṣṇam an-abhiṣyandi nāti-snigdham a-saṃkaram ।।

uṣṇodakopacārī syād brahma-cārī kṣapāśayaḥ ।
na vega-rodhī vyāyāma-krodha-śoka-himātapān ।।

pravāta-yāna-yānādhva-bhāṣyāty-āsana-saṃsthitīḥ ।
nīcāty-uccopadhānāhaḥ-svapna-dhūma-rajāṃsi ca ।।

-bhāṣyābhyāsana-saṃsthitīḥ -bhāṣyāty-aśana-saṃsthitīḥ 
-bhāṣyāty-āśana-saṃsthitīḥ
yāny ahāni pibet tāni tāvanty anyāny api tyajet ।
sarva-karmasv ayaṃ prāyo vyādhi-kṣīṇeṣu ca kramaḥ ।।

upacāras tu śamane kāryaḥ snehe virikta-vat ।
try-aham acchaṃ mṛdau koṣṭhe krūre sapta-dinaṃ pibet ।।

samyak-snigdho atha-vā yāvad ataḥ sātmyī-bhavet param ।
vātānulomyaṃ dīpto agnir varcaḥ snigdham a-saṃhatam ।।

snehodvegaḥ klamaḥ samyak-snigdhe rūkṣe viparyayaḥ ।
ati-snigdhe tu pāṇḍu-tvaṃ ghrāṇa-vaktra-guda-sravāḥ ।।

ṛdu-snigdhāṅga-tā glāniḥ nehodvego atha lāghavam nehodvego aṅga-lāghavam ti-snigdhe tu pāṇḍu-tva- i-malendriya-tā samyak- -ghrāṇa-vaktra-guda-sravāḥ -snigdhe 
rūkṣe viparyayaḥ
a-mātrayā-hito a-kāle mithyāhāra-vihārataḥ ।
snehaḥ karoti śophārśas-tandrā-stambha-vi-saṃjña-tāḥ ।।

kaṇḍū-kuṣṭha-jvarotkleśa-śūlānāha-bhramādikān ।
kṣut-tṛṣṇollekhana-sveda-rūkṣa-pānānna-bheṣajam ।।

-śūlānāha-bala-kṣayān ṣut-tṛṣṇollekhanaṃ svedo 
rūkṣaṃ pānānna-bheṣajam
takrāriṣṭa-khaloddāla-yava-śyāmāka-kodravāḥ ।
pippalī-tri-phalā-kṣaudra-pathyā-go-mūtra-guggulu ।।

akrāriṣṭaṃ khaloddāla- -yava-śyāmāka-kodravam
yathā-svaṃ prati-rogaṃ ca sneha-vyāpadi sādhanam ।
virūkṣaṇe laṅghana-vat kṛtāti-kṛta-lakṣaṇam ।।

snigdha-dravoṣṇa-dhanvottha-rasa-bhuk svedam ācaret ।
snigdhas try-ahaṃ sthitaḥ kuryād virekaṃ vamanaṃ punaḥ ।।

-rasa-bhuk svedam ācaran
ekāhaṃ dinam anyac ca kapham utkleśya tat-karaiḥ ।
māṃsalā medurā bhūri-śleṣmāṇo viṣamāgnayaḥ ।।

snehocitāś ca ye snehyās tān pūrvaṃ rūkṣayet tataḥ ।
saṃsnehya śodhayed evaṃ sneha-vyāpan na jāyate ।।

alaṃ malān īrayituṃ snehaś cā-sātmya-tāṃ gataḥ ।
bāla-vṛddhādiṣu sneha-parihārā-sahiṣṇuṣu ।।

yogān imān an-udvegān sadyaḥ-snehān prayojayet ।
prājya-māṃsa-rasās teṣu peyā vā sneha-bharjitā ।।

eyā vā sneha-bharjitāḥ
tila-cūrṇaś ca sa-sneha-phāṇitaḥ kṛśarā tathā ।
kṣīra-peyā ghṛtāḍhyoṣṇā dadhno vā sa-guḍaḥ saraḥ ।।

ila-cūrṇaṃ ca sa-sneha- -phāṇitaṃ kṛśarā tathā
peyā ca pañca-prasṛtā snehais taṇḍula-pañcamaiḥ ।
saptaite snehanāḥ sadyaḥ snehāś ca lavaṇolbaṇāḥ ।।

nehaś ca lavaṇolbaṇaḥ
tad dhy abhiṣyandy a-rūkṣaṃ ca sūkṣmam uṣṇaṃ vyavāyi ca ।
guḍānūpāmiṣa-kṣīra-tila-māṣa-surā-dadhi ।।

ad dhi viṣyandy a-rūkṣaṃ ca
kuṣṭha-śopha-prameheṣu snehārthaṃ na prakalpayet ।
tri-phalā-pippalī-pathyā-guggulv-ādi-vipācitān ।।

snehān yathā-svam eteṣāṃ yojayed a-vikāriṇaḥ ।
kṣīṇānāṃ tv āmayair agni-deha-saṃdhukṣaṇa-kṣamān ।।

ṣīṇānām āmayair agni-
dīptāntarāgniḥ pariśuddha-koṣṭhaḥ pratyagra-dhātur bala-varṇa-yuktaḥ ।
dṛḍhendriyo manda-jaraḥ śatāyuḥ snehopasevī puruṣaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ ।।

sūtrasthāna
svedas tāpopanāhoṣma-drava-bhedāc catur-vidhaḥ ।
tāpo agni-tapta-vasana-phāla-hasta-talādibhiḥ ।।

upanāho vacā-kiṇva-śatāhvā-devadārubhiḥ ।
dhānyaiḥ samastair gandhaiś ca rāsnairaṇḍa-jaṭāmiṣaiḥ ।।

udrikta-lavaṇaiḥ sneha-cukra-takra-payaḥ-plutaiḥ ।
kevale pavane śleṣma-saṃsṛṣṭe surasādibhiḥ ।।

pittena padmakādyais tu śālvaṇākhyaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
snigdhoṣṇa-vīryair mṛdubhiś carma-paṭṭair a-pūtibhiḥ ।।

ittena padmakādyaiś ca śālvalākhyaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ
a-lābhe vāta-jit pattra-kauśeyāvika-śāṭakaiḥ ।
baddhaṃ rātrau divā muñcen muñced rātrau divā-kṛtam ।।

ūṣmā tūtkārikā-loṣṭa-kapālopala-pāṃsubhiḥ ।
pattra-bhaṅgena dhānyena karīṣa-sikatā-tuṣaiḥ ।।

anekopāya-saṃtaptaiḥ prayojyo deśa-kālataḥ ।
śigru-vāraṇakairaṇḍa-karañja-surasārjakāt ।।

śirīṣa-vāsā-vaṃśārka-mālatī-dīrghavṛntataḥ ।
pattra-bhaṅgair vacādyaiś ca māṃsaiś cānūpa-vāri-jaiḥ ।।

daśa-mūlena ca pṛthak sahitair vā yathā-malam ।
sneha-vadbhiḥ surā-śukta-vāri-kṣīrādi-sādhitaiḥ ।।

kumbhīr galantīr nāḍīr vā pūrayitvā rujārditam ।
vāsasācchāditaṃ gātraṃ snigdhaṃ siñced yathā-sukham ।।

astrāvacchāditaṃ gātraṃ
tair eva vā dravaiḥ pūrṇaṃ kuṇḍaṃ sarvāṅga-ge anile ।
avagāhyāturas tiṣṭhed arśaḥ-kṛcchrādi-rukṣu ca ।।

nivāte antar-bahiḥ-snigdho jīrṇānnaḥ svedam ācaret ।
vyādhi-vyādhita-deśartu-vaśān madhya-varāvaram ।।

ir-vāte antar-bahiḥ-snigdho
kaphārto rūkṣaṇaṃ rūkṣo rūkṣaḥ snigdhaṃ kaphānile ।
āmāśaya-gate vāyau kaphe pakvāśayāśrite ।।

aphe taṃ rūkṣaṇai rūkṣo
rūkṣa-pūrvaṃ tathā sneha-pūrvaṃ sthānānurodhataḥ ।
alpaṃ vaṅkṣaṇayoḥ sv-alpaṃ dṛṅ-muṣka-hṛdaye na vā ।।

lpaṃ vaṅkṣaṇayoḥ svedaṃ
śīta-śūla-kṣaye svinno jāte aṅgānāṃ ca mārdave ।
syāc chanair mṛditaḥ snātas tataḥ sneha-vidhiṃ bhajet ।।

pittāsra-kopa-tṛṇ-mūrchā-svarāṅga-sadana-bhramāḥ ।
saṃdhi-pīḍā jvaraḥ śyāva-rakta-maṇḍala-darśanam ।।

svedāti-yogāc chardiś ca tatra stambhanam auṣadham ।
viṣa-kṣārāgny-atīsāra-cchardi-mohātureṣu ca ।।

svedanaṃ guru tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ prāyaḥ stambhanam anya-thā ।
drava-sthira-sara-snigdha-rūkṣa-sūkṣmaṃ ca bheṣajam ।।

svedanaṃ stambhanaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ rūkṣa-sūkṣma-sara-dravam ।
prāyas tiktaṃ kaṣāyaṃ ca madhuraṃ ca samāsataḥ ।।

stambhitaḥ syād bale labdhe yathoktāmaya-saṃkṣayāt ।
stambha-tvak-snāyu-saṃkoca-kampa-hṛd-vāg-ghanu-grahaiḥ ।।

pādauṣṭha-tvak-karaiḥ śyāvair ati-stambhitam ādiśet ।
na svedayed ati-sthūla-rūkṣa-dur-bala-mūrchitān ।।

stambhanīya-kṣata-kṣīṇa-kṣāma-madya-vikāriṇaḥ ।
timirodara-vīsarpa-kuṣṭha-śoṣāḍhya-rogiṇaḥ ।।

-kuṣṭha-śophāḍhya-rogiṇaḥ
pīta-dugdha-dadhi-sneha-madhūn kṛta-virecanān ।
bhraṣṭa-dagdha-guda-glāni-krodha-śoka-bhayārditān ।।

-krodha-śoka-bhayānvitān -krodha-rakta-kṣayānvitān
kṣut-tṛṣṇā-kāmalā-pāṇḍu-mehinaḥ pitta-pīḍitān ।
garbhiṇīṃ puṣpitāṃ sūtāṃ mṛdu cātyayike gade ।।

ṛdu tv ātyayike gade
śvāsa-kāsa-pratiśyāya-hidhmādhmāna-vibandhiṣu ।
svara-bhedānila-vyādhi-śleṣmāma-stambha-gaurave ।।

aṅga-marda-kaṭī-pārśva-pṛṣṭha-kukṣi-hanu-grahe ।
mahat-tve muṣkayoḥ khalyām āyāme vāta-kaṇṭake ।।

mūtra-kṛcchrārbuda-granthi-śukrāghātāḍhya-mārute ।
svedaṃ yathā-yathaṃ kuryāt tad-auṣadha-vibhāgataḥ ।।

svedo hitas tv an-āgneyo vāte medaḥ-kaphāvṛte ।
nivātaṃ gṛham āyāso guru-prāvaraṇaṃ bhayam ।।
upanāhāhava-krodhā bhūri-pānaṃ kṣudhātapaḥ ।।
ū̆upanāhāhava-krodha- ū̆-bhūri-pānaṃ kṣudhātapaḥ ū̆bv
bhūri-pāna-kṣud-ātapaḥ
svedayanti daśaitāni naram agni-guṇād ṛte ।।

sneha-klinnāḥ koṣṭha-gā dhātu-gā vā sroto-līnā ye ca śākhāsthi-saṃsthāḥ ।
doṣāḥ svedais te dravī-kṛtya koṣṭhaṃ nītāḥ samyak śuddhibhir nirhriyante ।।

sūtrasthāna
kaphe vidadhyād vamanaṃ saṃyoge vā kapholbaṇe ।
tad-vad virecanaṃ pitte viśeṣeṇa tu vāmayet ।।

nava-jvarātisārādhaḥ-pittāsṛg-rāja-yakṣmiṇaḥ ।
kuṣṭha-mehāpacī-granthi-ślīpadonmāda-kāsinaḥ ।।

śvāsa-hṛl-lāsa-vīsarpa-stanya-doṣordhva-rogiṇaḥ ।
a-vāmyā garbhiṇī rūkṣaḥ kṣudhito nitya-duḥkhitaḥ ।।

-stanya-rogordhva-rogiṇaḥ -vāmyā garbhiṇī-rūkṣa- 
-kṣudhitā nitya-duḥkhitāḥ
bāla-vṛddha-kṛśa-sthūla-hṛd-rogi-kṣata-dur-balāḥ ।
prasakta-vamathu-plīha-timira-kṛmi-koṣṭhinaḥ ।।

ūrdhva-pravṛtta-vāyv-asra-datta-vasti-hata-svarāḥ ।
mūtrāghāty udarī gulmī dur-vamo aty-agnir arśasaḥ ।।

ūrdhva-pravṛtta-vātāsra-
udāvarta-bhramāṣṭhīlā-pārśva-rug-vāta-rogiṇaḥ ।
ṛte viṣa-garā-jīrṇa-viruddhābhyavahārataḥ ।।

dāvarta-śramāṣṭhīlā-
prasakta-vamathoḥ pūrve prāyeṇāma-jvaro api ca ।
dhūmāntaiḥ karmabhir varjyāḥ sarvair eva tv a-jīrṇinaḥ ।।

vireka-sādhyā gulmārśo-visphoṭa-vyaṅga-kāmalāḥ ।
jīrṇa-jvarodara-gara-cchardi-plīha-halīmakāḥ ।।

īrṇa-jvarodara-cchardi- -plīhānāha-halīmakāḥ 
-plīha-pāṇḍu-halīmakāḥ
vidradhis timiraṃ kācaḥ syandaḥ pakvāśaya-vyathā ।
yoni-śukrāśrayā rogāḥ koṣṭha-gāḥ kṛmayo vraṇāḥ ।।

oni-śukra-gatā rogāḥ oni-śukrāśayā rogāḥ
vātāsram ūrdhva-gaṃ raktaṃ mūtrāghātaḥ śakṛd-grahaḥ ।
vāmyaś ca kuṣṭha-mehādyā na tu recyā nava-jvarī ।।

ātāsṛg ūrdhva-gaṃ raktaṃ a tu recyo nava-jvarī
alpāgny-adho-ga-pittāsra-kṣata-pāyv-atisāriṇaḥ ।
sa-śalyāsthāpita-krūra-koṣṭhāti-snigdha-śoṣiṇaḥ ।।

a-śalyābhihata-krūra-
atha sādhāraṇe kāle snigdha-svinnaṃ yathā-vidhi ।
śvo-vamyam utkliṣṭa-kaphaṃ matsya-māṣa-tilādibhiḥ ।।

atsya-māṃsa-tilādibhiḥ āṃsa-māṣa-tilādibhiḥ
niśāṃ suptaṃ su-jīrṇānnaṃ pūrvāhṇe kṛta-maṅgalam ।
nir-annam īṣat-snigdhaṃ vā peyayā pīta-sarpiṣam ।।

iśāṃ suptaṃ ca jīrṇānnaṃ
vṛddha-bālā-bala-klība-bhīrūn rogānurodhataḥ ।
ā-kaṇṭhaṃ pāyitān madyaṃ kṣīram ikṣu-rasaṃ rasam ।।

ā-kaṇṭhaṃ pāyayen madyaṃ
yathā-vikāra-vihitāṃ madhu-saindhava-saṃyutām ।
koṣṭhaṃ vibhajya bhaiṣajya-mātrāṃ mantrābhimantritām ।।

brahma-dakṣāśvi-rudrendra-bhū-candrārkānilānalāḥ ।
ṛṣayaḥ sauṣadhi-grāmā bhūta-saṃghāś ca pāntu vaḥ ।।

rasāyanam ivarṣīṇām a-marāṇām ivāmṛtam ।
sudhevottama-nāgānāṃ bhaiṣajyam idam astu te ।।

asāyanam ivarṣīṇāṃ evānām amṛtaṃ yathā namo bhaga-vate bhaiṣajya-gurave vaiḍūrya-prabha-rājāya ।।
tathā-gatāyārhate samyak-saṃbuddhāya ।।bhaiṣajye bhaiṣajye mahā-bhaiṣajye samudgate svāhā ।।
bhaiṣajye bhaiṣajye mahā-bhaiṣajye bhaiṣajya-samudgate svāhā 
bhaiṣajye mahā-bhaiṣajye samudgate svāhā
prāṅ-mukhaṃ pāyayet pīto muhūrtam anupālayet ।
tan-manā jāta-hṛl-lāsa-prasekaś chardayet tataḥ ।।

rāṅ-mukhaṃ pāyayet pītaṃ rāṅ-mukhaṃ pāyayet pīte 
-prasekaṃ chardayet tataḥ
aṅgulībhyām an-āyasto nālena mṛdunātha-vā ।
gala-tālv a-rujan vegān a-pravṛttān pravartayan ।।

ā-pravṛttān pravartayan ā-pravṛttān pravartayet 
a-pravṛttān pravartayet
pravartayan pravṛttāṃś ca jānu-tulyāsane sthitaḥ ।
ubhe pārśve lalāṭaṃ ca vamataś cāsya dhārayet ।।

prapīḍayet tathā nābhiṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ ca pratilomataḥ ।
kaphe tīkṣṇoṣṇa-kaṭukaiḥ pitte svādu-himair iti ।।

vamet snigdhāmla-lavaṇaiḥ saṃsṛṣṭe marutā kaphe ।
pittasya darśanaṃ yāvac chedo vā śleṣmaṇo bhavet ।।

hīna-vegaḥ kaṇā-dhātrī-siddhārtha-lavaṇodakaiḥ ।
vamet punaḥ punas tatra vegānām a-pravartanam ।।

pravṛttiḥ sa-vibandhā vā kevalasyauṣadhasya vā ।
a-yogas tena niṣṭhīva-kaṇḍū-koṭha-jvarādayaḥ ।।

nir-vibandhaṃ pravartante kapha-pittānilāḥ kramāt ।
samyag-yoge ati-yoge tu phena-candraka-rakta-vat ।।

hena-candrika-rakta-vat
manaḥ-prasādaḥ svāsthyaṃ cāvasthānaṃ ca svayaṃ bhavet ।
vaiparītyam a-yogānāṃ na cāti-mahatī vyathā ।।

manaḥ-prasādaḥ svāsthyaṃ ca avasthānaṃ svayaṃ 
bhavet
vamitaṃ kṣāma-tā dāhaḥ kaṇṭha-śoṣas tamo bhramaḥ ।
ghorā vāyv-āmayā mṛtyur jīva-śoṇita-nirgamāt ।।

samyag-yogena vamitaṃ kṣaṇam āśvāsya pāyayet ।
dhūma-trayasyānya-tamaṃ snehācāram athādiśet ।।

tataḥ sāyaṃ prabhāte vā kṣud-vān snātaḥ sukhāmbunā ।
bhuñjāno rakta-śāly-annaṃ bhajet peyādikaṃ kramam ।।

urāṇa-rakta-śālīnām huñjāno annam apekṣeta -sneha-lavaṇoṣaṇam eyādikam imaṃ kramam eyādikam imaṃ kramāt 
peyādikam amuṃ kramam
peyāṃ vilepīm a-kṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ ca yūṣaṃ rasaṃ trīn ubhayaṃ tathaikam ।
krameṇa seveta naro anna-kālān pradhāna-madhyāvara-śuddhi-śuddhaḥ ।।

yathāṇur agnis tṛṇa-go-mayādyaiḥ saṃdhukṣyamāṇo bhavati krameṇa ।
mahān sthiraḥ sarva-pacas tathaiva śuddhasya peyādibhir antarāgniḥ ।।

śuddhasya peyādibhir antar-agniḥ
jaghanya-madhya-pravare tu vegāś catvāra iṣṭā vamane ṣaḍ aṣṭau ।
daśaiva te dvi-tri-guṇā vireke prasthas tathā syād dvi-catur-guṇaś ca ।।

pittāvasānaṃ vamanaṃ virekād ardhaṃ kaphāntaṃ ca virekam āhuḥ ।
dvi-trān sa-viṭkān apanīya vegān meyaṃ vireke vamane tu pītam ।।

athainaṃ vāmitaṃ bhūyaḥ sneha-svedopapāditam ।
śleṣma-kāle gate jñātvā koṣṭhaṃ samyag virecayet ।।

bahu-pitto mṛduḥ koṣṭhaḥ kṣīreṇāpi viricyate ।
prabhūta-mārutaḥ krūraḥ kṛcchrāc chyāmādikair api ।।

kaṣāya-madhuraiḥ pitte virekaḥ kaṭukaiḥ kaphe ।
snigdhoṣṇa-lavaṇair vāyāv a-pravṛttau tu pāyayet ।।

uṣṇāmbu svedayed asya pāṇi-tāpena codaram ।
utthāne alpe dine tasmin bhuktvānye-dyuḥ punaḥ pibet ।।

a-dṛḍha-sneha-koṣṭhas tu pibed ūrdhvaṃ daśāhataḥ ।
bhūyo apy upaskṛta-tanuḥ sneha-svedair virecanam ।।

yaugikaṃ samyag ālocya smaran pūrvam atikramam ।
hṛt-kukṣy-a-śuddhir a-rucir utkleśaḥ śleṣma-pittayoḥ ।।

maran pūrvam anukramam
kaṇḍū-vidāhaḥ piṭikāh pīnaso vāta-viḍ-grahaḥ ।
a-yoga-lakṣaṇaṃ yogo vaiparītye yathoditāt ।।

aṇḍū-vidāhaḥ piṭikā
viṭ-pitta-kapha-vāteṣu niḥsṛteṣu kramāt sravet ।
niḥ-śleṣma-pittam udakaṃ śvetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sa-lohitam ।।

māṃsa-dhāvana-tulyaṃ vā medaḥ-khaṇḍābham eva vā ।
guda-niḥsaraṇaṃ tṛṣṇā bhramo netra-praveśanam ।।

śramo netra-praveśanam
bhavanty ati-viriktasya tathāti-vamanāmayāḥ ।
samyag-viriktam enaṃ ca vamanoktena yojayet ।।

dhūma-varjyena vidhinā tato vamita-vān iva ।
krameṇānnāni bhuñjāno bhajet prakṛti-bhojanam ।।

manda-vahnim a-saṃśuddham a-kṣāmaṃ doṣa-dur-balam ।
a-dṛṣṭa-jīrṇa-liṅgaṃ ca laṅghayet pīta-bheṣajam ।।

sneha-svedauṣadhotkleśa-saṅgair iti na bādhyate ।
saṃśodhanāsra-visrāva-sneha-yojana-laṅghanaiḥ ।।

yāty agnir manda-tāṃ tasmāt kramaṃ peyādim ācaret ।
srutālpa-pitta-śleṣmāṇaṃ madya-paṃ vāta-paittikam ।।

peyāṃ na pāyayet teṣāṃ tarpaṇādi-kramo hitaḥ ।
a-pakvaṃ vamanaṃ dośān pacyamānaṃ virecanam ।।

arpaṇādiḥ kramo hitaḥ arpaṇādiḥ kramo mataḥ 
tarpaṇādi-kramo mataḥ
nirhared vamanasyātaḥ pākaṃ na pratipālayet ।
dur-balo bahu-doṣaś ca doṣa-pākena yaḥ svayam ।।

viricyate bhedanīyair bhojyais tam upapādayet ।
dur-balaḥ śodhitaḥ pūrvam alpa-doṣaḥ kṛśo naraḥ ।।

hojyais taṃ samupācaret
a-parijñāta-koṣṭhaś ca piben mṛalpam auṣadham ।
varaṃ tad a-sakṛt-pītam anya-thā saṃśayāvaham ।।

araṃ tad a-sakṛt-pītaṃ ānya-thā saṃśayāvaham
hared bahūṃś calān doṣān alpān alpān punaḥ punaḥ ।
dur-balasya mṛdu-dravyair alpān saṃśamayet tu tān ।।

kleśayanti ciraṃ te hi hanyur vainam a-nirhṛtāḥ ।
mandāgniṃ krūra-koṣṭhaṃ ca sa-kṣāra-lavaṇair ghṛtaiḥ ।।

anyuś cainam a-nirhṛtāḥ
saṃdhukṣitāgniṃ vijita-kapha-vātaṃ ca śodhayet ।
rūkṣa-bahv-anila-krūra-koṣṭha-vyāyāma-śīlinām ।।

dīptāgnīnāṃ ca bhaiṣajyam a-virecyaiva jīryati ।
tebhyo vastiṃ purā dadyāt tataḥ snigdhaṃ virecanam ।।

ebhyo vastiṃ puro dadyāt
śakṛn nirhṛtya vā kiñ-cit tīkṣṇābhiḥ phala-vartibhiḥ ।
pravṛttaṃ hi malaṃ snigdho vireko nirharet sukham ।।

viṣābhighāta-piṭikā-kuṣṭha-śopha-visarpiṇaḥ ।
kāmalā-pāṇḍu-mehārtān nāti-snigdhān viśodhayet ।।

āti-snigdhān virecayet
sarvān sneha-virekaiś ca rūkṣais tu sneha-bhāvitān ।
karmaṇāṃ vamanādīnāṃ punar apy antare antare ।।

ūkṣaiś ca sneha-bhāvitān
sneha-svedau prayuñjīta sneham ante balāya ca ।
malo hi dehād utkleśya hriyate vāsaso yathā ।।

sneha-svedais tathotkliṣṭaḥ śodhyate śodhanair malaḥ ।
sneha-svedāv an-abhyasya kuryāt saṃśodhanaṃ tu yaḥ ।।

neha-svedais tathotkleśya riyate śodhanair malaḥ dāru śuṣkam ivān-āme śarīraṃ tasya dīryate ।।

buddhi-prasādaṃ balam indriyāṇāṃ dhātu-sthira-tvaṃ jvalanasya dīptim ।
cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti saṃśodhanaṃ samyag-upāsyamānam ।।

ū̆buddheḥ prasādaṃ balam indriyāṇāṃ ū̆dhātoḥ sthira-tvaṃ jvalanasya dīptim

sūtrasthāna
vātolbaṇeṣu doṣeṣu vāte vā vastir iṣyate ।
upakramāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ so agraṇīs tri-vidhas tu saḥ ।।

o agraṇīs tri-vidhaś ca saḥ
nirūho anvāsanaṃ vastir uttaras tena sādhayet ।
gulmānāha-khuḍa-plīha-śuddhātīsāra-śūlinaḥ ।।

jīrṇa-jvara-pratiśyāya-śukrānila-mala-grahān ।
vardhmāśmarī-rajo-nāśān dāruṇāṃś cānilāmayān ।।

an-āsthāpyās tv ati-snigdhaḥ kṣatorasko bhṛśaṃ kṛśaḥ ।
āmātīsārī vami-mān saṃśuddho datta-nāvanaḥ ।।

śvāsa-kāsa-prasekārśo-hidhmādhmānālpa-vahnayaḥ ।
śūna-pāyuḥ kṛtāhāro baddha-cchidrodakodarī ।।

addha-cchidra-dakodarī
kuṣṭhī ca madhu-mehī ca māsān sapta ca garbhiṇī ।
āsthāpyā eva cānvāsyā viśeṣād ati-vahnayaḥ ।।

rūkṣāḥ kevala-vātārtā nānuvāsyās ta eva ca ।
ye an-āsthāpyās tathā pāṇḍu-kāmalā-meha-pīnasāḥ ।।

nir-anna-plīha-viḍ-bhedi-guru-koṣṭha-kaphodarāḥ ।
abhiṣyandi-bhṛśa-sthūla-kṛmi-koṣṭhāḍhya-mārutāḥ ।।

-guru-koṣṭhaḥ kaphodarī bhiṣyandi-kṛśa-sthūla-
pīte viṣe gare apacyāṃ ślīpadī gala-gaṇḍa-vān ।
tayos tu netraṃ hemādi-dhātu-dārv-asthi-veṇu-jam ।।

go-pucchākāram a-cchidraṃ ślakṣṇarju guṭikā-mukham ।
ūne abde pañca pūrṇe asminn ā-saptabhyo aṅgulāni ṣaṭ ।।

saptame sapta tāny aṣṭau dvā-daśe ṣo-ḍaśe nava ।
dvā-daśaiva paraṃ viṃśād vīkṣya varṣāntareṣu ca ।।

vayo-bala-śarīrāṇi pramāṇam abhivardhayet ।
svāṅguṣṭhena samaṃ mūle sthaulyenāgre kaniṣṭhayā ।।

pūrṇe abde aṅgulam ādāya tad-ardhārdha-pravardhitam ।
try-aṅgulaṃ paramaṃ chidraṃ mūle agre vahate tu yat ।।

mudgaṃ māṣaṃ kalāyaṃ ca klinnaṃ karkandhukaṃ kramāt ।
mūla-cchidra-pramāṇena prānte ghaṭita-karṇikam ।।

vartyāgre pihitaṃ mūle yathā-svaṃ dvy-aṅgulāntaram ।
karṇikā-dvitayaṃ netre kuryāt tatra ca yojayet ।।

athā-svaṃ dvy-aṅgulāntare uryāt tatra prayojayet 
kuryāt tatra tu yojayet
ajāvi-mahiṣādīnāṃ vastiṃ su-mṛditaṃ dṛḍham ।
kaṣāya-raktaṃ niś-chidra-granthi-gandha-siraṃ tanum ।।

o-'jāvi-mahiṣādīnāṃ
grathitaṃ sādhu sūtreṇa sukha-saṃsthāpya-bheṣajam ।
vasty-a-bhāve aṅka-pādaṃ vā nyased vāso atha-vā ghanam ।।

ranthitaṃ sādhu sūtreṇa
nirūha-mātrā prathame prakuñco vatsare param ।
prakuñca-vṛddhiḥ praty-abdaṃ yāvat ṣaṭ prasṛtās tataḥ ।।

rakuñco vatsarāt param
prasṛtaṃ vardhayed ūrdhvaṃ dvā-daśāṣṭā-daśasya tu ।
ā-saptater idaṃ mānaṃ daśaiva prasṛtāḥ param ।।

vā-daśāṣṭā-daśasya ca
yathā-yathaṃ nirūhasya pādo mātrānuvāsane ।
āsthāpyaṃ snehitaṃ svinnaṃ śuddhaṃ labdha-balaṃ punaḥ ।।

anvāsanārhaṃ vijñāya pūrvam evānuvāsayet ।
śīte vasante ca divā rātrau ke-cit tato anya-dā ।।

ātrau ke-cit tato anya-thā
abhyakta-snātam ucitāt pāda-hīnaṃ hitaṃ laghu ।
a-snigdha-rūkṣam aśitaṃ sānu-pānaṃ dravādi ca ।।

ānu-pānaṃ dravādi vā
kṛta-caṅkramaṇaṃ mukta-viṇ-mūtraṃ śayane sukhe ।
nāty-ucchrite na coc-chīrṣe saṃviṣṭaṃ vāma-pārśvataḥ ।।

saṃkocya dakṣiṇaṃ sakthi prasārya ca tato aparam ।
athāsya netraṃ praṇayet snigdhe snigdha-mukhaṃ gude ।।

nigdhaṃ snigdha-mukhe gude
ucchvāsya vaster vadane baddhe hastam a-kampayan ।
pṛṣṭha-vaṃśaṃ prati tato nāti-druta-vilambitam ।।

nāti-vegaṃ na vā mandaṃ sakṛd eva prapīḍayet ।
sāvaśeṣaṃ ca kurvīta vāyuḥ śeṣe hi tiṣṭhati ।।

āvaśeṣaṃ prakurvīta
datte tūttāna-dehasya pāṇinā tāḍayet sphijau ।
tat-pārṣṇibhyāṃ tathā śayyāṃ pādataś ca trir utkṣipet ।।

tataḥ prasāritāṅgasya sopadhānasya pārṣṇike ।
āhanyān muṣṭināṅgaṃ ca snehenābhyajya mardayet ।।

vedanārtam iti sneho na hi śīghraṃ nivartate ।
yojyaḥ śīghraṃ nivṛtte anyaḥ sneho a-tiṣṭhann a-kārya-kṛt ।।

dīptāgniṃ tv āgata-snehaṃ sāyāhne bhojayel laghu ।
nivṛtti-kālaḥ paramas trayo yāmas tataḥ param ।।

aho-rātram upekṣeta parataḥ phala-vartibhiḥ ।
tīkṣṇair vā vastibhiḥ kuryād yatnaṃ sneha-nivṛttaye ।।

ati-raukṣyād an-āgacchan na cej jāḍyādi-doṣa-kṛt ।
upekṣetaiva hi tato adhyuṣitaś ca niśāṃ pibet ।।

prātar nāgara-dhānyāmbhaḥ koṣṇaṃ kevalam eva vā ।
anvāsayet tṛtīye ahni pañcame vā punaś ca tam ।।

yathā vā sneha-paktiḥ syād ato aty-ulbaṇa-mārutān ।
vyāyāma-nityān dīptāgnīn rūkṣāṃś ca prati-vāsaram ।।

ādhmāna-saṃkoca-purīṣa-bandha-kṣīṇendriya-tvā-ruci-bhaṅga-śūlāḥ ।
pāṅgulya-śākhāśrita-vāta-bhagna-bandhāś ca sādhyā hy anuvāsanena ।।

-vātāś ca sādhyā hy anuvāsanena
iti snehais tri-caturaiḥ snigdhe sroto-viśuddhaye ।
nirūhaṃ śodhanaṃ yuñjyād a-snigdhe snehanaṃ tanoḥ ।।

pañcame atha tṛtīye vā divase sādhake śubhe ।
madhyāhne kiñ-cid-āvṛtte prayukte bali-maṅgale ।।

abhyakta-sveditotsṛṣṭa-malaṃ nāti-bubhukṣitam ।
avekṣya puruṣaṃ doṣa-bheṣajādīni cādarāt ।।

vetya puruṣaṃ doṣa-
vastiṃ prakalpayed vaidyas tad-vidyair bahubhiḥ saha ।
kvāthayed viṃśati-palaṃ dravyasyāṣṭau phalāni ca ।।

ad-vedyair bahubhiḥ saha ad-vidhair bahubhiḥ saha
tataḥ kvāthāc caturthāṃśaṃ snehaṃ vāte prakalpayet ।
pitte svasthe ca ṣaṣṭhāṃśam aṣṭamāṃśaṃ kaphe adhike ।।

nehaṃ vāte anu kalpayet nehaṃ vāte tu kalpayet
sarva-tra cāṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ kalkād bhavati vā yathā ।
nāty-accha-sāndra-tā vasteḥ pala-mātraṃ guḍasya ca ।।

madhu-paṭv-ādi-śeṣaṃ ca yuktyā sarvaṃ tad ekataḥ ।
uṣṇāmbu-kumbhī-bāṣpeṇa taptaṃ khaja-samāhatam ।।

prakṣipya vastau praṇayet pāyau nāty-uṣṇa-śītalam ।
nāti-snigdhaṃ na vā rūkṣaṃ nāti-tīkṣṇaṃ na vā mṛdu ।।

nāty-accha-sāndraṃ nonāti-mātraṃ nā-paṭu nāti ca ।
lavaṇaṃ tad-vad amlaṃ ca paṭhanty anye tu tad-vidaḥ ।।

adanty anye tu tad-vidaḥ
mātrāṃ tri-palikāṃ kuryāt sneha-mākṣikayoḥ pṛthak ।
karṣārdhaṃ māṇimanthasya svasthe kalka-pala-dvayam ।।

sarva-dravāṇāṃ śeṣāṇāṃ palāni daśa kalpayet ।
mākṣikaṃ lavaṇaṃ snehaṃ kalkaṃ kvātham iti kramāt ।।

āvapeta nirūhāṇām eṣa saṃyojane vidhiḥ ।
uttāno datta-mātre tu nirūhe tan-manā bhavet ।।

kṛtopadhānaḥ sañjāta-vegaś cotkaṭakaḥ sṛjet ।
āgatau paramaḥ kālo muhūrto mṛtyave param ।।

-vegaś cotkaṭukaḥ sṛjet -vegaś cotkuṭakaḥ sṛjet 
muhūrto mṛtyave paraḥ
tatrānulomikaṃ sneha-kṣāra-mūtrāmla-kalpitam ।
tvaritaṃ snigdha-tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ vastim anyaṃ prapīḍayet ।।

atrānulomika-sneha-
vidadyāt phala-vartiṃ vā svedanottrāsanādi ca ।
svayam eva nivṛtte tu dvitīyo vastir iṣyate ।।

vedanotrāsanādi vā
tṛtīyo api caturtho api yāvad vā su-nirūḍha-tā ।
virikta-vac ca yogādīn vidyād yoge tu bhojayet ।।

āvad vā su-nirūha-tā idyād yoge tu yojayet
koṣṇena vāriṇā snātaṃ tanu-dhanva-rasaudanam ।
vikārā ye nirūḍhasya bhavanti pracalair malaiḥ ।।

oṣṇena vāriṇā snānaṃ ikārā ye nirūhasya
te sukhoṣṇāmbu-siktasya yānti bhukta-vataḥ śamam ।
atha vātārditaṃ bhūyaḥ sadya evānuvāsayet ।।

samyag-dhīnāti-yogāś ca tasya syuḥ sneha-pīta-vat ।
kiñ-cit-kālaṃ sthito yaś ca sa-purīṣo nivartate ।।

iñ-cit-kālaṃ sthito yasya
sānulomānilaḥ snehas tat siddham anuvāsanam ।
ekaṃ trīn vā balāse tu sneha-vastīn prakalpayet ।।

neha-vastīn prayojayet
pañca vā sapta vā pitte navaikā-daśa vānile ।
punas tato apy a-yugmāṃs tu punar āsthāpanaṃ tataḥ ।।

kapha-pittānileṣv annaṃ yūṣa-kṣīra-rasaiḥ kramāt ।
vāta-ghnauṣadha-niḥkvātha-trivṛtā-saindhavair yutaḥ ।।

vastir eko anile snigdhaḥ svādv-amloṣṇo rasānvitaḥ ।
nyagrodhādi-gaṇa-kvātha-padmakādi-sitā-yutau ।।

vādv-amloṣṇa-rasānvitaḥ
pitte svādu-himau sājya-kṣīrekṣu-rasa-mākṣikau ।
āragvadhādi-niḥkvātha-vatsakādi-yutās trayaḥ ।।

rūkṣāḥ sa-kṣaudra-go-mūtrās tīkṣṇoṣṇa-kaṭukāḥ kaphe ।
trayas te saṃnipāte api doṣān ghnanti yataḥ kramāt ।।

rayaś ca saṃnipāte api
tribhyaḥ paraṃ vastim ato necchanty anye cikitsakāḥ ।
na hi doṣaś caturtho asti punar dīyeta yaṃ prati ।।

ācārya-carakasyāto astis tribhyaḥ paraṃ mataḥ
utkleśanaṃ śuddhi-karaṃ doṣāṇāṃ śamanaṃ kramāt ।
tri-dhaiva kalpayed vastim ity anye api pracakṣate ।।

ri-dhaivaṃ kalpayed vastim
doṣauṣadhādi-balataḥ sarvam etat pramāṇayet ।
samyaṅ-nirūḍha-liṅgaṃ tu nā-saṃbhāvya nivartayet ।।

prāk sneha ekaḥ pañcānte dvā-daśāsthāpanāni ca ।
sānvāsanāni karmaivaṃ vastayas triṃśad īritāḥ ।।

kālaḥ pañca-daśaiko atra prāk sneho ante trayas tathā ।
ṣaṭ pañca-vasty-antaritā yogo aṣṭau vastayo atra tu ।।

trayo nirūhāḥ snehāś ca snehāv ādy-antayor ubhau ।
sneha-vastiṃ nirūhaṃ vā naikam evātiśīlayet ।।

utkleśāgni-vadhau snehān nirūhān maruto bhayam ।
tasmān nirūḍhaḥ snehyaḥ syān nirūhyaś cānuvāsitaḥ ।।

sneha-śodhana-yuktyaivaṃ vasti-karma tri-doṣa-jit ।
hrasvayā sneha-pānasya mātrayā yojitaḥ samaḥ ।।

mātrā-vastiḥ smṛtaḥ snehaḥ śīlanīyaḥ sadā ca saḥ ।
bāla-vṛddhādhva-bhāra-strī-vyāyāmāsakta-cintakaiḥ ।।

āla-vṛddhādhva-bhāṣya-strī-
vāta-bhagnā-balālpāgni-nṛpeśvara-sukhātmabhiḥ ।
doṣa-ghno niṣ-parīhāro balyaḥ sṛṣṭa-malaḥ sukhaḥ ।।

-nṛpaiśvarya-sukhātmabhiḥ
vastau rogeṣu nārīṇāṃ yoni-garbhāśayeṣu ca ।
dvi-trāsthāpana-śuddhebhyo vidadhyād vastim uttaram ।।

āturāṅgula-mānena tan-netraṃ dvā-daśāṅgulam ।
vṛttaṃ go-puccha-van mūla-madyayoḥ kṛta-karṇikam ।।

siddhārthaka-praveśāgraṃ ślakṣṇaṃ hemādi-saṃbhavam ।
kundāśvamāra-sumanaḥ-puṣpa-vṛntopamaṃ dṛḍham ।।

tasya vastir mṛdu-laghur mātrā śuktir vikalpya vā ।
atha snātāśītasyāsya sneha-vasti-vidhānataḥ ।।

ātrā śuktir vikalpya ca ātrā śuktiḥ prakalpya vā
ṛjoḥ sukhopaviṣṭasya pīṭhe jānu-same mṛdau ।
hṛṣṭe meḍhre sthite carjau śanaiḥ sroto-viśuddhaye ।।

sūkṣmāṃ śalākāṃ praṇayet tayā śuddhe anu-sevani ।
ā-mehanāntaṃ netraṃ ca niṣ-kampaṃ guda-vat tataḥ ।।

ayā śuddhe anu-sevanīm
pīḍite antar-gate snehe sneha-vasti-kramo hitaḥ ।
vastīn anena vidhinā dadyāt trīṃś caturo api vā ।।

īḍite anugate snehe
anuvāsana-vac cheṣaṃ sarvam evāsya cintayet ।
strīṇām ārtava-kāle tu yonir gṛhṇāty apāvṛteḥ ।।

vidadhīta tadā tasmād an-ṛtāv api cātyaye ।
yoni-vibhraṃśa-śūleṣu yoni-vyāpady asṛg-dare ।।

netraṃ daśāṅgulaṃ mudga-praveśaṃ catur-aṅgulam ।
apatya-mārge yojyaṃ syād dvy-aṅgulaṃ mūtra-vartmani ।।

mūtra-kṛcchra-vikāreṣu bālānāṃ tv ekam aṅgulam ।
prakuñco madhyamā mātrā bālānāṃ śuktir eva tu ।।

uttānāyāḥ śayānāyāḥ samyak saṃkocya sakthinī ।
ūrdhva-jānvās tri-caturān aho-rātreṇa yojayet ।।

vastīṃs tri-rātram evaṃ ca sneha-mātrāṃ vivardhayan ।
try-aham eva ca viśramya praṇidadhyāt punas try-aham ।।

neha-mātrāṃ vivardhayet
pakṣād vireko vamite tataḥ pakṣān nirūhaṇam ।
sadyo nirūḍhaś cānvāsyaḥ sapta-rātrād virecitaḥ ।।

yathā kusumbhādi-yutāt toyād rāgaṃ haret paṭaḥ ।
tathā dravī-kṛtād dehād vastir nirharate malān ।।

śākhā-gatāḥ koṣṭha-gatāś ca rogā marmordhva-sarvāvayavāṅga-jāś ca ।
ye santi teṣāṃ na tu kaś-cid anyo vāyoḥ paraṃ janmani hetur asti ।।

e santi teṣāṃ na hi kaś-cid anyo
viṭ-śleṣma-pittādi-maloccayānāṃ vikṣepa-saṃhāra-karaḥ sa yasmāt ।
tasyāti-vṛddhasya śamāya nānyad vaster vinā bheṣajam asti kiñ-cit ।।

iṭ-śleṣma-pittādi-malācayānāṃ iṭ-śleṣma-pittādi-malāśayānāṃ iṇ-mūtra-pittādi-malāśayānāṃ ikṣepa-saṃhāra-karo hi vāyuḥ 
asteḥ samaṃ bheṣajam asti yasmāt
tasmāc cikitsārdha iti pradiṣṭaḥ kṛtsnā cikitsāpi ca vastir ekaiḥ ।
tathā nijāgantu-vikāra-kāri-raktauṣadha-tvena sirā-vyadho api ।।

asmāc cikitsārdham iti pradiṣṭaḥ ṛtsnā cikitsāpi ca vastir eke

sūtrasthāna
ūrdhva-jatru-vikāreṣu viśeṣān nasyam iṣyate ।
nāsā hi śiraso dvāraṃ tena tad vyāpya hanti tān ।।

virecanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ ca śamanaṃ ca tri-dhāpi tat ।
virecanaṃ śiraḥ-śūla-jāḍya-syanda-galāmaye ।।

śamanaṃ ca tri-dhā bhavet marśa-dhmānāvapīḍākhyais tat punaḥ ṣaḍ-vidhaṃ smṛtam ।।

arśa-dhmānāvapīḍākhyāt
śopha-gaṇḍa-kṛmi-granthi-kuṣṭhāpasmāra-pīnase ।
bṛṃhaṇaṃ vāta-je śūle sūryāvarte svara-kṣaye ।।
snehena tīkṣṇaiḥ siddhena kalka-kvāthādibhiś ca tat ।।
nāsāsya-śoṣe vāk-saṅge kṛcchra-bodhe ava-bāhuke ।
śamanaṃ nīlikā-vyaṅga-keśa-doṣākṣi-rājiṣu ।।

-keśa-doṣākṣi-rogiṣu -keśa-doṣākṣi-roga-jit
yathā-svaṃ yaugikaiḥ snehair yathā-svaṃ ca prasādhitaiḥ ।
kalka-kvāthādibhiś cādyaṃ madhu-paṭv-āsavair api ।।

bṛṃhaṇaṃ dhanva-māṃsottha-rasāsṛk-khapurair api ।
śamanaṃ yojayet pūrvaiḥ kṣīreṇa salilena vā ।।

ṣīreṇa salilena ca ṣīreṇa ca jalena ca
marśaś ca pratimarśaś ca dvi-dhā sneho atra mātrayā ।
kalkādyair avapīḍas tu sa tīkṣṇair mūrdha-recanaḥ ।।

īkṣṇair mūrdha-virecanaḥ
dhmānaṃ virecanaś cūrṇo yuñjyāt taṃ mukha-vāyunā ।
ṣaḍ-aṅgula-dvi-mukhayā nāḍyā bheṣaja-garbhayā ।।

hmānaṃ virecanaiś cūrṇair āḍyā bhaiṣajya-garbhayā
sa hi bhūri-taraṃ doṣaṃ cūrṇa-tvād apakarṣati ।
pradeśiny-aṅgulī-parva-dvayān magna-samuddhṛtāt ।।

yāvat pataty asau bindur daśāṣṭau ṣaṭ krameṇa te ।
marśasyotkṛṣṭa-madhyonā mātrās tā eva ca kramāt ।।

bindu-dvayonāḥ kalkāder yojayen na tu nāvanam ।
toya-madya-gara-sneha-pītānāṃ pātum icchatām ।।

bhukta-bhakta-śiraḥ-snāta-snātu-kāma-srutāsṛjām ।
nava-pīnasa-vegārta-sūtikā-śvāsa-kāsinām ।।

huktābhyakta-śiraḥ-snāta-
śuddhānāṃ datta-vastīnāṃ tathān-ārtava-dur-dine ।
anya-trātyayikād vyādher atha nasyaṃ prayojayet ।।

prātaḥ śleṣmaṇi madhyāhne pitte sāyan-niśoś cale ।
svastha-vṛtte tu pūrvāhṇe śarat-kāla-vasantayoḥ ।।

śīte madhyan-dine grīṣme sāyaṃ varṣāsu sātape ।
vātābhibhūte śirasi hidhmāyām apatānake ।।

manyā-stambhe svara-bhraṃśe sāyaṃ prātar dine dine ।
ekāhāntaram anya-tra saptāhaṃ ca tad ācaret ।।

snigdha-svinnottamāṅgasya prāk-kṛtāvaśyakasya ca ।
nivāta-śayana-sthasya jatrūrdhvaṃ svedayet punaḥ ।।

athottānarju-dehasya pāṇi-pāde prasārite ।
kiñ-cid-unnata-pādasya kiñ-cin mūrdhani nāmite ।।

nāsā-puṭaṃ pidhāyaikaṃ paryāyeṇa niṣecayet ।
uṣṇāmbu-taptaṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ praṇāḍyā picunātha-vā ।।

raṇālyā picunātha-vā
datte pāda-tala-skandha-hasta-karṇādi mardayet ।
śanair ucchidya niṣṭhīvet pārśvayor ubhayos tataḥ ।।

śanair ucchindya niṣṭhīvet
ā-bheṣaja-kṣayād evaṃ dvis trir vā nasyam ācaret ।
mūrchāyāṃ śīta-toyena siñcet pariharan śiraḥ ।।

snehaṃ virecanasyānte dadyād doṣādy-apekṣayā ।
nasyānte vāk-śataṃ tiṣṭhed uttāno dhārayet tataḥ ।।

nehaṃ recana-nasyānte
dhūmaṃ pītvā kavoṣṇāmbu-kavaḍān kaṇṭha-śuddhaye ।
samyak-snigdhe sukhocchvāsa-svapna-bodhākṣa-pāṭavam ।।

rūkṣe akṣi-stabdha-tā śoṣo nāsāsye mūrdha-śūnya-tā ।
snigdhe ati kaṇḍū-guru-tā-prasekā-ruci-pīnasāḥ ।।

nigdhe ati kaṇḍūr guru-tā rasekā-ruci-pīnasāḥ
su-virikte akṣi-laghu-tā-vaktra-svara-viśuddhayaḥ ।
dur-virikte gadodrekaḥ kṣāma-tāti-virecite ।।

pratimarśaḥ kṣata-kṣāma-bāla-vṛddha-sukhātmasu ।
prayojyo a-kāla-varṣe api na tv iṣṭo duṣṭa-pīnase ।।

madya-pīte a-bala-śrotre kṛmi-dūṣita-mūrdhani ।
utkṛṣṭotkliṣṭa-doṣe ca hīna-mātra-tayā hi saḥ ।।

īna-māna-tayā hi saḥ
niśāhar-bhukta-vāntāhaḥ-svapnādhva-śrama-retasām ।
śiro-'bhyañjana-gaṇḍūṣa-prasrāvāñjana-varcasām ।।

danta-kāṣṭhasya hāsasya yojyo ante asau dvi-bindukaḥ ।
pañcasu srotasāṃ śuddhiḥ klama-nāśas triṣu kramāt ।।

dṛg-balaṃ pañcasu tato danta-dārḍhyaṃ maruc-chamaḥ ।
na nasyam ūna-saptābde nātītāśīti-vatsare ।।

na conāṣṭā-daśe dhūmaḥ kavaḍo nona-pañcame ।
na śuddhir ūna-daśame na cātikrānta-saptatau ।।

avaḍo nyūna-pañcame
ā-janma-maraṇaṃ śastaḥ pratimarśas tu vasti-vat ।
marśa-vac ca guṇān kuryāt sa hi nityopasevanāt ।।

na cātra yantraṇā nāpi vyāpadbhyo marśa-vad bhayam ।
tailam eva ca nasyārthe nityābhyāsena śasyate ।।

ailam eva ca nasyārthaṃ
śirasaḥ śleṣma-dhāma-tvāt snehāḥ svasthasya netare ।
āśu-kṛc-cira-kāri-tvaṃ guṇotkarṣāpakṛṣṭa-tā ।।

uṇotkṛṣṭāpakṛṣṭa-tā uṇotkṛṣṭāpakarṣa-tā 
guṇotkarṣāpakarṣa-tā
marśe ca pratimarśe ca viśeṣo na bhaved yadi ।
ko marśaṃ sa-parīhāraṃ sāpadaṃ ca bhajet tataḥ ।।

āpadaṃ ca vadet tataḥ
accha-pāna-vicārākhyau kuṭī-vātātapa-sthitī ।
anvāsa-mātrā-vastī ca tad-vad eva vinirdiśet ।।

ad-vad eva ca nirdiśet
paṭola-mudga-vārtāka-hrasvamūlaka-jāṅgalaiḥ ।
rasaiḥ śāli-yavān adyān nasya-karmaṇi ṣaḍ-vidhe ।।

uccair-bhāṣaṇam āyāsam a-jīrṇā-sātmya-bhojanam ।
datta-nasyo naraḥ krodhaṃ yānādīṃś ca vivarjayet ।।
jīvantī-jala-devadāru-jalada-tvak-sevya-gopī-himaṃ ।।dārvī-tvaṅ-madhuka-plavāguru-varī-puṇḍrāhva-bilvotpalam ।।dhāvanyau surabhiṃ sthire kṛmiharaṃ pattraṃ truṭīṃ reṇukāṃ ।।kiñjalkaṃ kamalād balāṃ śata-guṇe divye ambhasi kvāthayet ।।
tailād rasaṃ daśa-guṇaṃ pariśeṣya tena tailaṃ paceta salilena daśaiva vārān । pāke kṣipec ca daśame samam āja-dugdhaṃ nasyaṃ mahā-guṇam uśanty aṇu-tailam etat ।।

ailaṃ pacec ca salilena daśaiva vārān
ghanonnata-prasanna-tvak-skandha-grīvāsya-vakṣasaḥ ।
dṛḍhendriyāsta-palitā bhaveyur nasya-śīlinaḥ ।।

ṛḍhendriyās tv a-palitā

sūtrasthāna
jatrūrdhva-kapha-vātottha-vikārāṇām a-janmane ।
ucchedāya ca jātānāṃ pibed dhūmaṃ sadātma-vān ।।

atrūrdhvaṃ kapha-vātottha-
snigdho madhyaḥ sa tīkṣṇaś ca vāte vāta-kaphe kaphe ।
yojyo na rakta-pittārti-viriktodara-mehiṣu ।।

ojyo na pitta-raktārta- ojyo na pitta-raktārti-
timirordhvānilādhmāna-rohiṇī-datta-vastiṣu ।
matsya-madya-dadhi-kṣīra-kṣaudra-sneha-viṣāśiṣu ।।

śirasy abhihate pāṇḍu-roge jāgarite niśi ।
rakta-pittāndhya-bādhirya-tṛṇ-mūrchā-mada-moha-kṛt ।।

dhūmo a-kāle ati-pīto vā tatra śīto vidhir hitaḥ ।
kṣuta-jṛmbhita-viṇ-mūtra-strī-sevā-śastra-karmaṇām ।।

-strī-sevā-śastra-karmiṇām
hāsasya danta-kāṣṭhasya dhūmam ante piben mṛdum ।
kāleṣv eṣu niśāhāra-nāvanānte ca madhyamam ।।

āsyasya danta-kāṣṭhasya
nidrā-nasyāñjana-snāna-ccharditānte virecanam ।
vasti-netra-sama-dravyaṃ tri-kośaṃ kārayed ṛju ।।

mūlāgre aṅguṣṭha-kolāsthi-praveśaṃ dhūma-netrakam ।
tīkṣṇa-snehana-madhyeṣu trīṇi catvāri pañca ca ।।

ūle agre aṅguṣṭha-kolāsthi-
aṅgulānāṃ kramāt pātuḥ pramāṇenāṣṭakāni tat ।
ṛjūpaviṣṭas tac-cetā vivṛtāsyas tri-paryayam ।।

ṛjūpaviṣṭas tac-citto
pidhāya cchidram ekaikaṃ dhūmaṃ nāsikayā pibet ।
prāk piben nāsayotkliṣṭe doṣe ghrāṇa-śiro-gate ।।

oṣe nāsā-śiro-gate
utkleśanārthaṃ vaktreṇa viparītaṃ tu kaṇṭha-ge ।
mukhenaivodvamed dhūmaṃ nāsayā dṛg-vighāta-kṛt ।।

ākṣepa-mokṣaiḥ pātavyo dhūmas tu tris tribhis tribhiḥ ।
ahnaḥ pibet sakṛt snigdhaṃ dvir madhyaṃ śodhanaṃ param ।।

hūmas trīṃs trīṃs tribhis tribhiḥ
triś catur vā mṛdau tatra dravyāṇy aguru guggulu ।
musta-sthauṇeya-śaileya-naladośīra-vālakam ।।

riś catur vā mṛdos tatra
varāṅga-kauntī-madhuka-bilva-majjailavālukam ।
śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarja-raso dhyāmakaṃ madanaṃ plavam ।।

śallakī kuṅkumaṃ māṣā yavāḥ kundurukas tilāḥ ।
snehaḥ phalānāṃ sārāṇāṃ medo majjā vasā ghṛtam ।।

śamane śallakī lākṣā pṛthvīkā kamalotpalam ।
nyagrodhodumbarāśvattha-plakṣa-lodhra-tvacaḥ sitā ।।

yaṣṭīmadhu suvarṇatvak padmakaṃ raktayaṣṭikā ।
gandhāś cā-kuṣṭha-tagarās tīkṣṇe jyotiṣmatī niśā ।।

daśa-mūla-manohvālaṃ lākṣā śvetā phala-trayam ।
gandha-dravyāṇi tīkṣṇāni gaṇo mūrdha-virecanaḥ ।।

aśa-mūla-manohvāla- -lākṣā śvetā phala-trayam
jale sthitām aho-rātram iṣīkāṃ dvā-daśāṅgulām ।
piṣṭair dhūmauṣadhair evaṃ pañca-kṛtvaḥ pralepayet ।।

iṣṭair dhūmauṣadhair eva
vartir aṅguṣṭhaka-sthūlā yava-madhyā yathā bhavet ।
chāyā-śuṣkāṃ vi-garbhāṃ tāṃ snehābhyaktāṃ yathā-yatham ।।

artir aṅguṣṭha-vat sthūlā
dhūma-netrārpitāṃ pātum agni-pluṣṭāṃ prayojayet ।
śarāva-saṃpuṭa-cchidre nāḍīṃ nyasya daśāṅgulām ।।
aṣṭāṅgulāṃ vā vaktreṇa kāsa-vān dhūmam āpibet ।।
kāsaḥ śvāsaḥ pīnaso vi-svara-tvaṃ pūtir gandhaḥ pāṇḍu-tā keśa-doṣaḥ ।
karṇāsyākṣi-srāva-kaṇḍv-arti-jāḍyaṃ tandrā hidhmā dhūma-paṃ na spṛśanti ।।

hṛt-kaṇṭhendriya-saṃśuddhir lāghavaṃ śirasaḥ śamaḥ ।
yatheritānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ samyak-pītasya lakṣaṇam ।।

sūtrasthāna
catuḥ-prakāro gaṇḍūṣaḥ snigdhaḥ śamana-śodhanau ।
ropaṇaś ca trayas tatra triṣu yojyāś calādiṣu ।।

antyo vraṇa-ghnaḥ snigdho atra svādv-amla-paṭu-sādhitaiḥ ।
snehaiḥ saṃśamanas tikta-kaṣāya-madhurauṣadhaiḥ ।।

śodhanas tikta-kaṭv-amla-paṭūṣṇai ropaṇaḥ punaḥ ।
kaṣāya-tiktakais tatra snehaḥ kṣīraṃ madhūdakam ।।

śuktaṃ madyaṃ raso mūtraṃ dhānyāmlaṃ ca yathā-yatham ।
kalkair yuktaṃ vipakvaṃ vā yathā-sparśaṃ prayojayet ।।

danta-harṣe danta-cāle mukha-roge ca vātike ।
sukhoṣṇam atha-vā śītaṃ tila-kalkodakaṃ hitam ।।

gaṇḍūṣa-dhāraṇe nityaṃ tailaṃ māṃsa-raso atha-vā ।
ūṣā-dāhānvite pāke kṣate cāgantu-saṃbhave ।।

ṣate vāgantu-saṃbhave
viṣe kṣārāgni-dagdhe ca sarpir dhāryaṃ payo atha-vā ।
vaiśadyaṃ janayaty āśu saṃdadhāti mukhe vraṇān ।।

iṣa-kṣārāgni-dagdhe ca aiśadyaṃ janayaty āsye 
saṃdadhāti mukha-vraṇān
dāha-tṛṣṇā-praśamanaṃ madhu-gaṇḍūṣa-dhāraṇam ।
dhānyāmlam āsya-vairasya-mala-daurgandhya-nāśanam ।।

tad evā-lavaṇaṃ śītaṃ mukha-śoṣa-haraṃ param ।
āśu kṣārāmbu-gaṇḍūṣo bhinatti śleṣmaṇaś cayam ।।

sukhoṣṇodaka-gaṇḍūṣair jāyate vaktra-lāghavam ।
nivāte sātape svinna-mṛdita-skandha-kandharaḥ ।।

gaṇḍūṣam a-piban kiñ-cid-unnatāsyo vidhārayet ।
kapha-pūrṇāsya-tā yāvat sravad-ghrāṇākṣa-tātha-vā ।।
a-saṃcāryo mukhe pūrṇe gaṇḍūṣaḥ kavaḍo anya-thā ।।
ū̆a-saṃcāryo mukhe a-pūrṇe
manyā-śiraḥ-karṇa-mukhākṣi-rogāḥ praseka-kaṇṭhāmaya-vaktra-śoṣāḥ ।
hṛl-lāsa-tandrā-ruci-pīnasāś ca sādhyā viśeṣāt kavaḍa-graheṇa ।।
kalko rasa-kriyā cūrṇas tri-vidhaṃ pratisāraṇam ।।
alko rasa-kriyā cūrṇaṃ
yuñjyāt tat kapha-rogeṣu gaṇḍūṣa-vihitauṣadhaiḥ ।
mukhālepas tri-dhā doṣa-viṣa-hā varṇa-kṛc ca saḥ ।।

ukha-lepas tri-dhā doṣa-
vyādher apacayaḥ puṣṭir vaiśadyaṃ vaktra-lāghavam ।
indriyāṇāṃ prasādaś ca kavaḍe śuddhi-lakṣaṇam ।।

hīnāj jāḍya-kaphotkleśāv a-rasa-jñānam eva ca ।
ati-yogān mukhe pākaḥ śoṣa-tṛṣṇā-ruci-klamaḥ ।।

īnād dhmāna-kaphotleśāv
uṣṇo vāta-kaphe śastaḥ śeṣeṣv aty-artha-śītalaḥ ।
tri-pramāṇaś catur-bhāga-tri-bhāgārdhāṅgulonnatiḥ ।।

a-śuṣkasya sthitis tasya śuṣko dūṣayati cchavim ।
tam ārdrayitvāpanayet tad-ante abhyaṅgam ācaret ।।

vivarjayed divā-svapna-bhāṣyāgny-ātapa-śuk-krudhaḥ ।
na yojyaḥ pīnase a-jīrṇe datta-nasye hanu-grahe ।।

atte nasye hanu-grahe
a-rocake jāgarite sa tu hanti su-yojitaḥ ।
a-kāla-palita-vyaṅga-valī-timira-nīlikāḥ ।।

a ca hanti su-yojitaḥ
kola-majjā vṛṣān mūlaṃ śābaraṃ gaura-sarṣapāḥ ।
siṃhī-mūlaṃ tilāḥ kṛṣṇā dārvī-tvaṅ nis-tuṣā yavāḥ ।।

darbha-mūla-himośīra-śirīṣa-miśi-taṇḍulāḥ ।
kumudotpala-kalhāra-dūrvā-madhuka-candanam ।।

kālīyaka-tilośīra-māṃsī-tagara-padmakam ।
tālīśa-gundrā-puṇḍrāhva-yaṣṭī-kāśa-natāguru ।।

ity ardhārdhoditā lepā hemantādiṣu ṣaṭ smṛtāḥ ।
-mukhālepana-śīlānāṃ dṛḍhaṃ bhavati darśanam ।।

vadanaṃ cā-parimlānaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ tāmarasopamam ।
abhyaṅga-seka-picavo vastiś ceti catur-vidham ।।

mūrdha-tailaṃ bahu-guṇaṃ tad vidyād uttarottaram ।
tatrābhyaṅgaḥ prayoktavyo raukṣya-kaṇḍū-malādiṣu ।।

ūkṣa-kaṇḍū-malādiṣu
arūṃṣikā-śiras-toda-dāha-pāka-vraṇeṣu tu ।
pariṣekaḥ picuḥ keśa-śāta-sphuṭana-dhūpane ।।

-dāha-pāka-vraṇeṣu ca
netra-stambhe ca vastis tu prasupty-ardita-jāgare ।
nāsāsya-śoṣe timire śiro-roge ca dāruṇe ।।

vidhis tasya niṣaṇṇasya pīṭhe jānu-same mṛdau ।
śuddhākta-svinna-dehasya dinānte gavya-māhiṣam ।।

dvā-daśāṅgula-vistīrṇaṃ carma-paṭṭaṃ śiraḥ-samam ।
ā-karṇa-bandhana-sthānaṃ lalāṭe vastra-veṣṭite ।।

caila-veṇikayā baddhvā māṣa-kalkena lepayet ।
tato yathā-vyādhi śṛtaṃ snehaṃ koṣṇaṃ niṣecayet ।।

ūrdhvaṃ keśa-bhuvo yāvad aṅgulaṃ dhārayec ca tam ।
ā-vaktra-nāsikotkledād daśāṣṭau ṣaṭ calādiṣu ।।

ā-vaktra-nāsikā-kledād
mātrā-sahasrāṇy a-ruje tv ekaṃ skandhādi mardayet ।
mukta-snehasya paramaṃ saptāhaṃ tasya sevanam ।।

aptāhaṃ tasya secanam
dhārayet pūraṇaṃ karṇe karṇa-mūlaṃ vimardayan ।
rujaḥ syān mārdavaṃ yāvan mātrā-śatam a-vedane ।।

arṇa-mūlaṃ vimardayet
yāvat paryeti hastāgraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ jānu-maṇḍalam ।
nimeṣonmeṣa-kālena samaṃ mātrā tu sā smṛtā ।।

imeṣonmeṣa-mātreṇa
kaca-sadana-sita-tva-piñjara-tvaṃ pariphuṭanaṃ śirasaḥ samīra-rogān ।
jayati janayatīndriya-prasādaṃ svara-hanu-mūrdha-balaṃ ca mūrdha-tailam ।।

aca-śadana-sita-tva-piñjara-tvaṃ aca-śadana-sita-tva-piñjara-tva- aca-sadana-sita-tva-piñjara-tva-

sūtrasthāna
sarveṣām akṣi-rogāṇām ādāv āścyotanaṃ hitam ।
ruk-toda-kaṇḍu-gharṣāśru-dāha-rāga-nibarhaṇam ।।

-dāha-roga-nibarhaṇam
uṣṇaṃ vāte kaphe koṣṇaṃ tac chītaṃ rakta-pittayoḥ ।
nivāta-sthasya vāmena pāṇinonmīlya locanam ।।

śuktau pralambayānyena picu-vartyā kanīnike ।
daśa dvā-daśa vā bindūn dvy-aṅgulād avasecayet ।।

tataḥ pramṛjya mṛdunā cailena kapha-vātayoḥ ।
anyena koṣṇa-pānīya-plutena svedayen mṛdu ।।

aty-uṣṇa-tīkṣṇaṃ rug-rāga-dṛṅ-nāśāyākṣi-secanam ।
ati-śītaṃ tu kurute nistoda-stambha-vedanāḥ ।।

kaṣāya-vartma-tāṃ gharṣaṃ kṛcchrād unmeṣaṇaṃ bahu ।
vikāra-vṛddhim aty-alpaṃ saṃrambham a-parisrutam ।।

gatvā saṃdhi-śiro-ghrāṇa-mukha-srotāṃsi bheṣajam ।
ūrdhva-gān nayane nyastam apavartayate malān ।।

atvā saṃdhi-sirā-ghrāṇa-
athāñjanaṃ śuddha-tanor netra-mātrāśraye male ।
pakva-liṅge alpa-śophāti-kaṇḍū-paicchilya-lakṣite ।।

akva-liṅge alpa-śophārti-
manda-gharṣāśru-rāge akṣṇi prayojyaṃ ghana-dūṣike ।
ārte pitta-kaphāsṛgbhir mārutena viśeṣataḥ ।।

lekhanaṃ ropaṇaṃ dṛṣṭi-prasādanam iti tri-dhā ।
añjanaṃ lekhanaṃ tatra kaṣāyāmla-paṭūṣaṇaiḥ ।।

ropaṇaṃ tiktakair dravyaiḥ svādu-śītaiḥ prasādanam ।
tīkṣṇāñjanābhisaṃtapte nayane tat prasādanam ।।

prayujyamānaṃ labhate pratyañjana-samāhvayam ।
daśāṅgulā tanur madhye śalākā mukulānanā ।।

praśastā lekhane tāmrī ropaṇe kāla-loha-jā ।
aṅgulī ca suvarṇotthā rūpya-jā ca prasādane ।।

piṇḍo rasa-kriyā cūrṇas tri-dhaivāñjana-kalpanā ।
gurau madhye laghau doṣe tāṃ krameṇa prayojayet ।।

uru-madhya-laghau doṣe āḥ krameṇa prayojayet
piṇḍasya tīkṣṇa-dravyasya mṛdu-dravya-kṛtasya ca ।
hareṇu-mātraṃ dvi-guṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ kathayanty api ।।

rasa-kriyāyām apy evaṃ viḍaṅga-phala-mātrakam ।
śalākāṃ dvi-guṇāṃ tīkṣṇe cūrṇe ca tri-guṇāṃ mṛdau ।।

hareṇu-mātrā piṇḍasya vella-mātrā rasa-kriyā ।
tīkṣṇasya dvi-guṇaṃ tasya mṛdunaś cūrṇitasya ca ।।

iṇḍo hareṇu-mātras tu areṇu-mātraṃ piṇḍasya areṇu-mātraḥ piṇḍas tu 
alla-mātrā rasa-kriyā ṛdoś cūrṇāñjanasya ca
dve śalāke tu tīkṣṇasya tisras tad-itarasya ca ।
niśi svapne na madhyāhne mlāne noṣṇa-gabhastibhiḥ ।।

israḥ syur itarasya ca iśi svapnena madhyāhne 
pānānnoṣṇa-gabhastibhiḥ
akṣi-rogāya doṣāḥ syur vardhitotpīḍita-drutāḥ ।
prātaḥ sāyaṃ ca tac-chāntyai vy-abhre arke ato añjayet sadā ।।

vadanty anye tu na divā prayojyaṃ tīkṣṇam añjanam ।
vireka-dur-balaṃ cakṣur ādityaṃ prāpya sīdati ।।

svapnena rātrau kālasya saumya-tvena ca tarpitā ।
śīta-sātmyā dṛg āgneyī sthira-tāṃ labhate punaḥ ।।

aty-udrikte balāse tu lekhanīye atha-vā gade ।
kāmam ahny api nāty-uṣṇe tīkṣṇam akṣṇi prayojayet ।।

aśmano janma lohasya tata eva ca tīkṣṇa-tā ।
upaghāto api tenaiva tathā netrasya tejasaḥ ।।

na rātrāv api śīte ati netre tīkṣṇāñjanaṃ hitam ।
doṣam a-srāvayet stabdhaṃ kaṇḍū-jāḍyādi-kāri tat ।।

oṣam a-srāvayat stabdhaṃ oṣam a-srāvayat stambha- 
oṣaṃ na srāvayet stambha- -kaṇḍū-jāḍyādi-kāri tat
nāñjayed bhīta-vamita-viriktāśita-vegite ।
kruddha-jvarita-tāntākṣi-śiro-ruk-śoka-jāgare ।।

a-dṛṣṭe arke śiraḥ-snāte pītayor dhūma-madyayoḥ ।
a-jīrṇe agny-arka-saṃtapte divā-supte pipāsite ।।

ivā-svapne pipāsite
ati-tīkṣṇa-mṛdu-stoka-bahv-accha-ghana-karkaśam ।
aty-artha-śītalaṃ taptam añjanaṃ nāvacārayet ।।

ty-arthaṃ śītalaṃ taptam
athānumīlayan dṛṣṭim antaḥ saṃcārayec chanaiḥ ।
añjite vartmanī kiñ-cic cālayec caivam añjanam ।।

tīkṣṇaṃ vyāpnoti sahasā na conmeṣa-nimeṣaṇam ।
niṣpīḍanaṃ ca vartmabhyāṃ kṣālanaṃ vā samācaret ।।

apetauṣadha-saṃrambhaṃ nirvṛtaṃ nayanaṃ yadā ।
vyādhi-doṣartu-yogyābhir adbhiḥ prakṣālayet tadā ।।

dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhakenākṣi tato vāmaṃ sa-vāsasā ।
ūrdhva-vartmani saṃgṛhya śodhyaṃ vāmena cetarat ।।

vartma-prāpto añjanād doṣo rogān kuryād ato anya-thā ।
kaṇḍū-jāḍye añjanaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ dhūmaṃ vā yojayet punaḥ ।।

artma-prāptāñjanād doṣo ogān kuryāt tato anya-thā tīkṣṇāñjanābhitapte tu cūrṇaṃ pratyañjanaṃ himam ।।

ū̆tīkṣṇāñjanāti-tapte tu ū̆tīkṣṇāñjanāti-yoge tu ū̆cūrṇaṃ pratyañjanaṃ hitam

sūtrasthāna
nayane tāmyati stabdhe śuṣke rūkṣe abhighātite ।
vāta-pittāture jihme śīrṇa-pakṣmāvilekṣaṇe ।।

kṛcchronmīla-sirā-harṣa-sirotpāta-tamo-'rjunaiḥ ।
syanda-manthānyato-vāta-vāta-paryāya-śukrakaiḥ ।।

āture śānta-rāgāśru-śūla-saṃrambha-dūṣike ।
nivāte tarpaṇaṃ yojyaṃ śuddhayor mūrdha-kāyayoḥ ।।

kāle sādhāraṇe prātaḥ sāyaṃ vottāna-śāyinaḥ ।
yava-māṣa-mayīṃ pālīṃ netra-kośād bahiḥ samām ।।

āyaṃ cottāna-śāyinaḥ
dvy-aṅguloccāṃ dṛḍhāṃ kṛtvā yathā-svaṃ siddham āvapet ।
sarpir nimīlite netre taptāmbu-pravilāyitam ।।

aptāmbu-pravilāpitam
naktāndhya-vāta-timira-kṛcchra-bodhādike vasām ।
ā-pakṣmāgrād athonmeṣaṃ śanakais tasya kurvataḥ ।।

mātrā vigaṇayet tatra vartma-saṃdhi-sitāsite ।
dṛṣṭau ca krama-śo vyādhau śataṃ trīṇi ca pañca ca ।।

ātrāṃ vigaṇayet tatra
śatāni sapta cāṣṭau ca daśa manthe daśānile ।
pitte ṣaṭ svastha-vṛtte ca balāse pañca dhārayet ।।

aśa manthe anile daśa
kṛtvāpāṅge tato dvāraṃ snehaṃ pātre nigālayet ।
pibec ca dhūmaṃ nekṣeta vyoma rūpaṃ ca bhāsvaram ।।

yoma rūpaṃ ca bhās-karam
itthaṃ prati-dinaṃ vāyau pitte tv ekāntaraṃ kaphe ।
svasthe tu dvy-antaraṃ dadyād ā-tṛpter iti yojayet ।।

prakāśa-kṣama-tā svāsthyaṃ viśadaṃ laghu locanam ।
tṛpte viparyayo a-tṛpte ati-tṛpte śleṣma-jā rujaḥ ।।

ṛpte ati śleṣma-jā rujaḥ
sneha-pītā tanur iva klāntā dṛṣṭir hi sīdati ।
tarpaṇān-antaraṃ tasmād dṛg-balādhāna-kāriṇam ।।

puṭa-pākaṃ prayuñjīta pūrvokteṣv eva yakṣmasu ।
sa vāte snehanaḥ śleṣma-sahite lekhano hitaḥ ।।

ūrvokteṣv eṣu yakṣmasu ūrvokteṣu ca yakṣmasu
dṛg-daurbalye anile pitte rakte svasthe prasādanaḥ ।
bhū-śaya-prasahānūpa-medo-majja-vasāmiṣaiḥ ।।

snehanaṃ payasā piṣṭair jīvanīyaiś ca kalpayet ।
mṛga-pakṣi-yakṛn-māṃsa-muktāyas-tāmra-saindhavaiḥ ।।

sroto-ja-śaṅkha-phenālair lekhanaṃ mastu-kalkitaiḥ ।
mṛga-pakṣi-yakṛn-majja-vasāntra-hṛdayāmiṣaiḥ ।।

madhuraiḥ sa-ghṛtaiḥ stanya-kṣīra-piṣṭaiḥ prasādanam ।
bilva-mātraṃ pṛthak piṇḍaṃ māṃsa-bheṣaja-kalkayoḥ ।।

urubūka-vaṭāmbho-ja-pattraiḥ snehādiṣu kramāt ।
veṣṭayitvā mṛdā liptaṃ dhava-dhanvana-go-mayaiḥ ।।

-pattraiḥ snigdhādiṣu kramāt
pacet pradīptair agny-ābhaṃ pakvaṃ niṣpīḍya tad-rasam ।
netre tarpaṇa-vad yuñjyāt śataṃ dve trīṇi dhārayet ।।

lekhana-snehanāntyeṣu koṣṇau pūrvau himo aparaḥ ।
dhūma-po ante tayor eva yogās tatra ca tṛpti-vat ।।

tarpaṇaṃ puṭa-pākaṃ ca nasyān-arhe na yojayet ।
yāvanty ahāni yuñjīta dvis tato hita-bhāg bhavet ।।
mālatī-mallikā-puṣpair baddhākṣo nivasen niśām ।।
ū̆baddhākṣo nivasen niśi
sarvātmanā netra-balāya yatnaṃ kurvīta nasyāñjana-tarpaṇādyaiḥ ।
dṛṣṭiś ca naṣṭā vividhaṃ jagac ca tamo-mayaṃ jāyata eka-rūpam ।।

sūtrasthāna
nānā-vidhānāṃ śalyānāṃ nānā-deśa-prabodhinām ।
āhartum abhyupāyo yas tad yantraṃ yac ca darśane ।।

ānā-deśa-vibādhinām
arśo-bhagandarādīnāṃ śastra-kṣārāgni-yojane ।
śeṣāṅga-parirakṣāyāṃ tathā vasty-ādi-karmaṇi ।।

ghaṭikālābu-śṛṅgaṃ ca jāmbavauṣṭhādikāni ca ।
aneka-rūpa-kāryāṇi yantrāṇi vividhāny ataḥ ।।

vikalpya kalpayet buddhyā yathā-sthūlaṃ tu vakṣyate ।
tulyāni kaṅka-siṃharkṣa-kākādi-mṛga-pakṣiṇām ।।

mukhair mukhāni yantrāṇāṃ kuryāt tat-saṃjñakāni ca ।
aṣṭā-daśāṅgulāyāmāny āyasāni ca bhūri-śaḥ ।।

masūrākāra-pary-antaiḥ kaṇṭhe baddhāni kīlakaiḥ ।
vidyāt svastika-yantrāṇi mūle aṅkuśa-natāni ca ।।

ūle aṅkuśa-nibhāni ca
tair dṛḍhair asthi-saṃlagna-śalyāharaṇam iṣyate ।
kīla-baddha-vimuktāgrau saṃdaṃśau ṣo-ḍaśāṅgulau ।।

tvak-sirā-snāyu-piśita-lagna-śalyāpakarṣaṇau ।
ṣaḍ-aṅgulo anyo haraṇe sūkṣma-śalyopa-pakṣmaṇām ।।

mucuṇḍī sūkṣma-dantarjur mūle rucaka-bhūṣaṇā ।
gambhīra-vraṇa-māṃsānām armaṇaḥ śeṣitasya ca ।।

ucuṭī sūkṣma-dantarjur
dve dvā-daśāṅgule matsya-tāla-vat dvy-eka-tālake ।
tāla-yantre smṛte karṇa-nāḍī-śalyāpahāriṇī ।।

-tālu-vat dvy-eka-tāluke ālu-yantre smṛte karṇa- 
-nāḍī-śalyāpahāraṇe -nāḍī-śalyāpakarṣaṇī
nāḍī-yantrāṇi suṣirāṇy ekāneka-mukhāni ca ।
sroto-gatānāṃ śalyānām āmayānāṃ ca darśane ।।

kāneka-mukhāni tu
kriyāṇāṃ su-kara-tvāya kuryād ācūṣaṇāya ca ।
tad-vistāra-parīṇāha-dairghyaṃ sroto-'nurodhataḥ ।।

daśāṅgulārdha-nāhāntaḥ-kaṇṭha-śalyāvalokinī ।
nāḍī pañca-mukha-cchidrā catuṣ-karṇasya saṃgrahe ।।

-kaṇṭha-śalyāvalokane
vāraṅgasya dvi-karṇasya tri-cchidrā tat-pramāṇataḥ ।
vāraṅga-karṇa-saṃsthānānāha-dairghyānurodhataḥ ।।

nāḍīr evaṃ-vidhāś cānyā draṣṭuṃ śalyāni kārayet ।
padma-karṇikayā mūrdhni sadṛśī dvā-daśāṅgulā ।।

caturtha-suṣirā nāḍī śalya-nirghātinī matā ।
arśasāṃ go-stanākāraṃ yantrakaṃ catur-aṅgulam ।।

nāhe pañcāṅgulaṃ puṃsāṃ pramadānāṃ ṣaḍ-aṅgulam ।
dvi-cchidraṃ darśane vyādher eka-cchidraṃ tu karmaṇi ।।

madhye asya try-aṅgulaṃ chidram aṅguṣṭhodara-vistṛtam ।
ardhāṅgulocchritodvṛtta-karṇikaṃ ca tad-ūrdhvataḥ ।।

-karṇikaṃ tu tad-ūrdhvataḥ
śamy-ākhyaṃ tādṛg a-cchidraṃ yantram arśaḥ-prapīḍanam ।
sarva-thāpanayed oṣṭhaṃ chidrād ūrdhvaṃ bhagandare ।।

ghrāṇārbudārśasām eka-cchidrā nāḍy-aṅgula-dvayā ।
pradeśinī-parīṇāhā syād bhagandara-yantra-vat ।।

aṅgulī-trāṇakaṃ dāntaṃ vārkṣaṃ vā catur-aṅgulam ।
dvi-cchidraṃ go-stanākāraṃ tad-vaktra-vivṛtau sukham ।।

yoni-vraṇekṣaṇaṃ madhye suṣiraṃ ṣo-ḍaśāṅgulam ।
mudrā-baddhaṃ catur-bhittam ambho-ja-mukulānanam ।।

udrā-baddhaṃ catur-bhinnam udrā-baddhaṃ catuṣ-koṇam
catuḥ-śalākam ākrāntaṃ mūle tad vikasen mukhe ।
yantre nāḍī-vraṇābhyaṅga-kṣālanāya ṣaḍ-aṅgule ।।

vasti-yantrākṛtī mūle mukhe aṅguṣṭha-kalāya-khe ।
agrato a-karṇike mūle nibaddha-mṛdu-carmaṇī ।।

dvi-dvārā nalikā piccha-nalikā vodakodare ।
dhūma-vasty-ādi-yantrāṇi nirdiṣṭāni yathā-yatham ।।

try-aṅgulāsyaṃ bhavec chṛṅgaṃ cūṣaṇe aṣṭā-daśāṅgulam ।
agre siddhārthaka-cchidraṃ su-naddhaṃ cūcukākṛti ।।

syād dvā-daśāṅgulo alābur nāhe tv aṣṭā-daśāṅgulaḥ ।
catus-try-aṅgula-vṛttāsyo dīpto antaḥ śleṣma-rakta-hṛt ।।

tad-vad ghaṭī hitā gulma-vilayonnamane ca sā ।
śalākākhyāni yantrāṇi nānā-karmākṛtīni ca ।।

ānā-karmākṛtīni tu
yathā-yoga-pramāṇāni teṣām eṣaṇa-karmaṇī ।
ubhe gaṇḍū-pada-mukhe srotobhyaḥ śalya-hāriṇī ।।

eṣām eṣaṇa-karmaṇi
masūra-dala-vaktre dve syātām aṣṭa-navāṅgule ।
śaṅkavaḥ ṣaḍ ubhau teṣāṃ ṣo-ḍaśa-dvā-daśāṅgulau ।।

vyūhane ahi-phaṇā-vaktrau dvau daśa-dvā-daśāṅgulau ।
cālane śara-puṅkhāsyāv āhārye baḍiśākṛtī ।।

nato agre śaṅkunā tulyo garbha-śaṅkur iti smṛtaḥ ।
aṣṭāṅgulāyatas tena mūḍha-garbhaṃ haret striyāḥ ।।

aśmary-āharaṇaṃ sarpa-phaṇā-vad vakram agrataḥ ।
śara-puṅkha-mukhaṃ danta-pātanaṃ catur-aṅgulam ।।

śmary-āharaṇe sarpa- -phaṇā-vad vaktram agrataḥ
kārpāsa-vihitoṣṇīṣāḥ śalākāḥ ṣaṭ pramārjane ।
pāyāv āsanna-dūrārthe dve daśa-dvā-daśāṅgule ।।

dve ṣaṭ-saptāṅgule ghrāṇe dve karṇe aṣṭa-navāṅgule ।
karṇa-śodhanam aśvattha-pattra-prāntaṃ sruvānanam ।।

śalākā-jāmbavauṣṭhānāṃ kṣāre agnau ca pṛthak trayam ।
yuñjyāt sthūlāṇu-dīrghāṇāṃ śalākām antra-vardhmani ।।

madhyordhva-vṛtta-daṇḍāṃ ca mūle cārdhendu-saṃnibhām ।
kolāsthi-dala-tulyāsyā nāsārśo-'rbuda-dāha-kṛt ।।

aṣṭāṅgulā nimna-mukhās tisraḥ kṣārauṣadha-krame ।
kanīnī-madhyamānāmī-nakha-māna-samair mukhaiḥ ।।

aniṣṭhā-madhyamānāmī-
svaṃ svam uktāni yantrāṇi meḍhra-śuddhy-añjanādiṣu ।
anu-yantrāṇy ayas-kānta-rajjū-vastrāśma-mudgarāḥ ।।

ṇu-yantrāṇy ayas-kānta-
vadhrāntra-jihvā-vālāś ca śākhā-nakha-mukha-dvi-jāḥ ।
kālaḥ pākaḥ karaḥ pādo bhayaṃ harṣaś ca tat-kriyāḥ ।।

adhry-antra-jihvā-vālāś ca ardhrāntra-jihvā-vālāś ca v
-śākhā-nakha-mukha-dvi-jāḥ
upāya-vit pravibhajed ālocya nipuṇaṃ dhiyā ।।

nirghātanonmathana-pūraṇa-mārga-śuddhi-saṃvyūhanāharaṇa-bandhana-pīḍanāni ।
ācūṣaṇonnamana-nāmana-cāla-bhaṅga-vyāvartanarju-karaṇāni ca yantra-karma ।।

vivartate sādhv avagāhate ca grāhyaṃ gṛhītvoddharate ca yasmāt ।
yantreṣv ataḥ kaṅka-mukhaṃ pradhānaṃ sthāneṣu sarveṣv adhikāri yac ca ।।

ū̆nivartate sādhv avagāhate ca ū̆sthāneṣu sarveṣv a-vikāri yac ca

sūtrasthāna
ṣaḍ-viṃśatiḥ su-karmārair ghaṭitāni yathā-vidhi ।
śastrāṇi roma-vāhīni bāhulyenāṅgulāni ṣaṭ ।।

su-rūpāṇi su-dhārāṇi su-grahāṇi ca kārayet ।
a-karālāni su-dhmāta-su-tīkṣṇāv artite ayasi ।।

samāhita-mukhāgrāṇi nīlāmbho-ja-cchavīni ca ।
nāmānugata-rūpāṇi sadā saṃnihitāni ca ।।

svonmānārdha-caturthāṃśa-phalāny ekaika-śo api ca ।
prāyo dvi-trāṇi yuñjīta tāni sthāna-viśeṣataḥ ।।

va-mānārdha-caturthāṃśa-
maṇḍalāgraṃ vṛddhi-pattram utpalādhy-ardha-dhārake ।
sarpaiṣaṇyau vetasākhyaṃ śarāry-āsya-tri-kūrcake ।।

kuśāsyaṃ sāṭa-vadanam antar-vaktrārdha-candrake ।
vrīhi-mukhaṃ kuṭhārī ca śalākāṅguli-śastrake ।।

kuśāsyā sāṭa-vadanā antar-vaktrārdha-candrakam channa-vaktrārdha-candrake 
channa-vaktrārdha-candrakam
baḍiśaṃ kara-pattrākhyaṃ kartarī nakha-śastrakam ।
danta-lekhanakaṃ sūcyaḥ kūrco nāma khajāhvayam ।।

ārā catur-vidhākārā tathā syāt karṇa-vedhanī ।।
tathā syāt karṇa-vedhanam
maṇḍalāgraṃ phale teṣāṃ tarjany-antar-nakhākṛti ।
lekhane chedane yojyaṃ pothakī-śuṇḍikādiṣu ।।

aṇḍalāgraṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ
vṛddhi-pattraṃ kṣurākāraṃ cheda-bhedana-pāṭane ।
ṛjv-agram unnate śophe gambhīre ca tad anya-thā ।।

ambhīre tu tato anya-thā
natāgraṃ pṛṣṭhato dīrgha-hrasva-vaktraṃ yathāśrayam ।
utpalādhy-ardha-dhārākhye bhedane chedane tathā ।।

-hrasva-vaktraṃ yathāśayam -hrasva-vaktraṃ yathā-kramam 
-hrasva-vaktraṃ yathā-yatham -hrasva-vaktre yathā-yatham
sarpāsyaṃ ghrāṇa-karṇārśaś-chedane ardhāṅgulaṃ phale ।
gater anveṣaṇe ślakṣṇā gaṇḍū-pada-mukhaiṣaṇī ।।

bhedanārthe aparā sūcī-mukhā mūla-niviṣṭa-khā ।
vetasaṃ vyadhane srāvye śarāry-āsya-tri-kūrcake ।।

kuśāṭā-vadane srāvye dvy-aṅgulaṃ syāt tayoḥ phalam ।
tad-vad antar-mukhaṃ tasya phalam adhy-ardham aṅgulam ।।

c kuśāṭā vadane srāvye
ardha-candrānanaṃ caitat tathādhy-ardhāṅgulaṃ phale ।
vrīhi-vaktraṃ prayojya ca tat sirodarayor vyadhe ।।

pṛthuḥ kuṭhārī go-danta-sadṛśārdhāṅgulānanā ।
tayordhva-daṇḍayā vidhyed upary asthnāṃ sthitāṃ sirām ।।

tāmrī śalākā dvi-mukhī mukhe kurubakākṛtiḥ ।
liṅga-nāśaṃ tayā vidhyet kuryād aṅguli-śastrakam ।।

āmrī śalākā dvi-mukhā
mudrikā-nirgata-mukhaṃ phale tv ardhāṅgulāyatam ।
yogato vṛddhi-pattreṇa maṇḍalāgreṇa vā samam ।।

tat pradeśiny-agra-parva-pramāṇārpaṇa-mudrikam ।
