sūtra-baddhaṃ gala-sroto-roga-cchedana-bhedane ।।

-pramāṇārpita-mudrikam
grahaṇe śuṇḍikārmāder baḍiśaṃ su-natānanam ।
chede asthnāṃ karapattraṃ tu khara-dhāraṃ daśāṅgulam ।।

aḍiśaḥ su-natānanaḥ
vistāre dvy-aṅgulaṃ sūkṣma-dantaṃ su-tsaru-bandhanam ।
snāyu-sūtra-kaca-cchede kartarī kartarī-nibhā ।।

vakrarju-dhāraṃ dvi-mukhaṃ nakha-śastraṃ navāṅgulam ।
sūkṣma-śalyoddhṛti-ccheda-bheda-pracchāna-lekhane ।।

-bheda-pracchanna-lekhane
eka-dhāraṃ catuṣ-koṇaṃ prabaddhākṛti caikataḥ ।
danta-lekhanakaṃ tena śodhayed danta-śarkarām ।।

ravṛddhākṛti caikataḥ
vṛttā gūḍha-dṛḍhāḥ pāśe tisraḥ sūcyo atra sīvane ।
māṃsalānāṃ pradeśānāṃ try-aśrā try-aṅgulam āyatā ।।

alpa-māṃsāsthi-saṃdhi-stha-vraṇānāṃ dvy-aṅgulāyatā ।
vrīhi-vaktrā dhanur-vakrā pakvāmāśaya-marmasu ।।

sā sārdha-dvy-aṅgulā sarva-vṛttās tāś catur-aṅgulāḥ ।
kūrco vṛttaika-pīṭha-sthāḥ saptāṣṭau vā su-bandhanāḥ ।।

ā sārdha-dvy-aṅgulā sarvā ṛttās tāś catur-aṅgulāḥ
sa yojyo nīlikā-vyaṅga-keśa-śāteṣu kuṭṭane ।
ardhāṅgula-mukhair vṛttair aṣṭābhiḥ kaṇṭakaiḥ khajaḥ ।।

-keśa-śātana-kuṭṭane
pāṇibhyāṃ mathyamānena ghrāṇāt tena hared asṛk ।
vyadhanaṃ karṇa-pālīnāṃ yūthikā-mukulānanam ।।

yadhane karṇa-pālīnāṃ ūthikā-mukulānanā
ārārdhāṅgula-vṛttāsyā tat-praveśā tathordhvataḥ ।
catur-aśrā tayā vidhyec chophaṃ pakvāma-saṃśaye ।।

karṇa-pālīṃ ca bahalāṃ bahalāyāś ca śasyate ।
sūcī tri-bhāga-suṣirā try-aṅgulā karṇa-vedhanī ।।

asyā eva ca śasyate
jalaukaḥ-kṣāra-dahana-kācopala-nakhādayaḥ ।
a-lauhāny anu-śastrāṇi tāny evaṃ ca vikalpayet ।।

aparāṇy api yantrādīny upayogaṃ ca yaugikam ।
utpāṭya-pāṭya-sīvyaiṣya-lekhya-pracchāna-kuṭṭanam ।।

tpāṭya-pāṭya-sevyaiṣya- -lekhya-pracchanna-kuṭṭanam
chedyaṃ bhedyaṃ vyadho mantho graho dāhaś ca tat-kriyāḥ ।
kuṇṭha-khaṇḍa-tanu-sthūla-hrasva-dīrgha-tva-vakra-tāḥ ।।

śastrāṇāṃ khara-dhāra-tvam aṣṭau doṣāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
cheda-bhedana-lekhyārthaṃ śastraṃ vṛnta-phalāntare ।।

tarjanī-madhyamāṅguṣṭhair gṛhṇīyāt su-samāhitaḥ ।
visrāvaṇāni vṛntāgre tarjany-aṅguṣṭhakena ca ।।

tala-pracchanna-vṛntāgraṃ grāhyaṃ vrīhi-mukhaṃ mukhe ।
mūleṣv āharaṇārthāni kriyā-saukaryato aparam ।।

ūleṣv āharaṇārthe tu ūleṣv āharaṇārtheṣu
syān navāṅgula-vistāraḥ su-ghano dvā-daśāṅgulaḥ ।
kṣauma-pattrorṇa-kauśeya-dukūla-mṛdu-carma-jaḥ ।।

vinyasta-pāśaḥ su-syūtaḥ sāntarorṇā-stha-śastrakaḥ ।
śalākā-pihitāsyaś ca śastra-kośaḥ su-saṃcayaḥ ।।

jalaukasas tu sukhināṃ rakta-srāvāya yojayet ।
duṣṭāmbu-matsya-bhekāhi-śava-kotha-malodbhavāḥ ।।

uṣṭāmbu-matsya-bhekādi-
raktāḥ śvetā bhṛśaṃ kṛṣṇāś capalāḥ sthūla-picchilāḥ ।
indrāyudha-vicitrordhva-rājayo romaśāś ca tāḥ ।।

sa-viṣā varjayet tābhiḥ kaṇḍū-pāka-jvara-bhramāḥ ।
viṣa-pittāsra-nut kāryaṃ tatra śuddhāmbu-jāḥ punaḥ ।।

iṣa-pittāsra-jit kāryaṃ atra śuddhāmbu-saṃbhavāḥ
nir-viṣāḥ śaivala-śyāvā vṛttā nīlordhva-rājayaḥ ।
kaṣāya-pṛṣṭhās tanv-aṅgyaḥ kiñ-cit-pītodarāś ca yāḥ ।।

tā apy a-samyag-vamanāt pratataṃ ca nipātanāt ।
sīdantiḥ salilaṃ prāpya rakta-mattā iti tyajet ।।

īdanti salilaṃ prāpya
athetarā niśā-kalka-yukte ambhasi pariplutāḥ ।
avanti-some takre vā punaś cāśvāsitā jale ।।

āñjike kālaśeye vā
lāgayed ghṛta-mṛt-stanya-rakta-śastra-nipātanaiḥ ।
pibantīr unnata-skandhāś chādayen mṛdu-vāsasā ।।

āgayet pala-mṛt-stanya-
saṃpṛktād duṣṭa-śuddhāsrāj jalaukā duṣṭa-śoṇitam ।
ādatte prathamaṃ haṃsaḥ kṣīraṃ kṣīrodakād iva ।।

aṃsṛṣṭād duṣṭa-śuddhāsrāj
gulmārśo-vidradhīn kuṣṭha-vāta-rakta-galāmayān ।
netra-rug-viṣa-vīsarpān śamayanti jalaukasaḥ ।।

daṃśasya tode kaṇḍvāṃ vā mokṣayed vāmayec ca tām ।
paṭu-tailākta-vadanāṃ ślakṣṇa-kaṇḍana-rūṣitām ।।

okṣayed vāmayec ca tāḥ aṭu-tailākta-vadanāḥ ślakṣṇa-kaṇḍana-rūkṣitām 
ślakṣṇa-kaṇḍana-rūṣitāḥ ślakṣṇa-kaṇḍana-rūkṣitāḥ
rakṣan rakta-madād bhūyaḥ saptāhaṃ tā na pātayet ।
pūrva-vat paṭu-tā dārḍhyaṃ samyag-vānte jalaukasām ।।

klamo ati-yogān mṛtyur vā dur-vānte stabdha-tā madaḥ ।
anya-trānya-tra tāḥ sthāpyā ghaṭe mṛtsnāmbu-garbhiṇi ।।

lālādi-kotha-nāśārthaṃ sa-viṣāḥ syus tad-anvayāt ।
a-śuddhau srāvayed daṃśān haridrā-guḍa-mākṣikaiḥ ।।

śata-dhautājya-picavas tato lepāś ca śītalāḥ ।
duṣṭa-raktāpagamanāt sadyo rāga-rujāṃ śamaḥ ।।

a-śuddhaṃ calitaṃ sthānāt sthitaṃ raktaṃ vraṇāśaye ।
vy-amlī-bhavet paryuṣitaṃ tasmāt tat srāvayet punaḥ ।।

mlī-bhavet paryuṣitaṃ
yuñjyān nālābu-ghaṭikā rakte pittena dūṣite ।
tāsām anala-saṃyogād yuñjyāt tu kapha-vāyunā ।।

uñjyāc ca kapha-vāyunā
kaphena duṣṭaṃ rudhiraṃ na śṛṅgeṇa vinirharet ।
skanna-tvād vāta-pittābhyāṃ duṣṭaṃ śṛṅgeṇa nirharet ।।

a śṛṅgeṇāti nirharet a śṛṅgeṇābhinirharet
gātraṃ baddhvopari dṛḍhaṃ rajjvā paṭṭena vā samam ।
snāyu-saṃdhy-asthi-marmāṇi tyajan pracchānam ācaret ।।

adho-deśa pravisṛtaiḥ padair upari-gāmibhiḥ ।
na gāḍha-ghana-tiryagbhir na pade padam ācaran ।।

a pade padam ācaret
pracchānenaika-deśa-sthaṃ grathitaṃ jala-janmabhiḥ ।
harec chṛṅgādibhiḥ suptam asṛg vyāpi sirā-vyadhaiḥ ।।

ranthitaṃ jala-janmabhiḥ
pracchānaṃ piṇḍite vā syād avagāḍhe jalaukasaḥ ।
tvak-sthe alābu-ghaṭī-śṛṅgaṃ siraiva vyāpake asṛji ।।

vātādi-dhāma vā śṛṅga-jalauko-'lābubhiḥ kramāt ।
srutāsṛjaḥ pradehādyaiḥ śītaiḥ syād vāyu-kopataḥ ।।
sa-toda-kaṇḍuḥ śophas taṃ sarpiṣoṣṇena secayet ।।
ū̆sa-toda-kaṇḍū-śophas taṃ

sūtrasthāna
madhuraṃ lavaṇaṃ kiñ-cid a-śītoṣṇam a-saṃhatam ।
padmendragopa-hemāvi-śaśa-lohita-lohitam ।।

lohitaṃ prabhavaḥ śuddhaṃ tanos tenaiva ca sthitaḥ ।
tat pitta-śleṣmalaiḥ prāyo dūṣyate kurute tataḥ ।।

ohitaṃ pravadec chuddhaṃ
visarpa-vidradhi-plīha-gulmāgni-sadana-jvarān ।
mukha-netra-śiro-roga-mada-tṛḍ-lavaṇāsya-tāḥ ।।

kuṣṭha-vātāsra-pittāsra-kaṭv-amlodgiraṇa-bhramān ।
śītoṣṇa-snigdha-rūkṣādyair upakrāntāś ca ye gadāḥ ।।

samyak sādhyā na sidhyanti te ca rakta-prakopa-jāḥ ।
teṣu srāvayituṃ raktam udriktaṃ vyadhayet sirām ।।

na tūna-ṣo-ḍaśātīta-saptaty-abda-srutāsṛjām ।
a-snigdhā-sveditāty-artha-sveditānila-rogiṇām ।।

a nyūna-ṣo-ḍaśātīta-
garbhiṇī-sūtikā-jīrṇa-pittāsra-śvāsa-kāsinām ।
atīsārodara-cchardi-pāṇḍu-sarvāṅga-śophinām ।।

sneha-pīte prayukteṣu tathā pañcasu karmasu ।
nā-yantritāṃ sirāṃ vidhyen na tiryaṅ nāpy an-utthitām ।।

a tiryaṅ nāpy an-ucchritām
nāti-śītoṣṇa-vātābhreṣv anya-trātyayikād gadāt ।
śiro-netra-vikāreṣu lalāṭyāṃ mokṣayet sirām ।।

ālāṭyāṃ mokṣayet sirām ālāṭyā mokṣayet sirāḥ 
lalāṭyā mokṣayet sirāḥ
apāṅgyām upanāsyāṃ vā karṇa-rogeṣu karṇa-jām ।
nāsā-rogeṣu nāsāgre sthitāṃ nāsā-lalāṭayoḥ ।।

pāṅgyā upanāsyā vā
pīnase mukha-rogeṣu jihvauṣṭha-hanu-tālu-gāḥ ।
jatrūrdhva-granthiṣu grīvā-karṇa-śaṅkha-śiraḥ-śritāḥ ।।

atrūrdhvaṃ granthiṣu grīvā-
uro-'pāṅga-lalāṭa-sthā unmāde apasmṛtau punaḥ ।
hanu-saṃdhau samaste vā sirāṃ bhrū-madhya-gāminīm ।।

ro-'pāṅga-lalāṭa-sthām irā bhrū-madhya-gāminīḥ
vidradhau pārśva-śūle ca pārśva-kakṣā-stanāntare ।
tṛtīyake aṃsayor madhye skandhasyādhaś caturthake ।।

pravāhikāyāṃ śūlinyāṃ śroṇito dvy-aṅgule sthitām ।
śukra-meḍhrāmaye meḍhra ūru-gāṃ gala-gaṇḍayoḥ ।।

gṛdhrasyāṃ jānuno adhas-tād ūrdhvaṃ vā catur-aṅgule ।
indra-vaster adho apacyāṃ dvy-aṅgule catur-aṅgule ।।

ūrdhvaṃ gulphasya sakthy-artau tathā kroṣṭuka-śīrṣake ।
pāda-dāhe khuḍe harṣe vipādyāṃ vāta-kaṇṭake ।।

ūrdhvaṃ gulphasya saṃdhy-artau
cipye ca dvy-aṅgule vidhyed upari kṣipra-marmaṇaḥ ।
gṛdhrasyām iva viśvācyāṃ yathoktānām a-darśane ।।

marma-hīne yathāsanne deśe anyāṃ vyadhayet sirām ।
atha snigdha-tanuḥ sajja-sarvopakaraṇo balī ।।

kṛta-svasty-ayanaḥ snigdha-rasānna-pratibhojitaḥ ।
agni-tāpātapa-svinno jānūccāsana-saṃsthitaḥ ।।

mṛdu-paṭṭātta-keśānto jānu-sthāpita-kūrparaḥ ।
muṣṭibhyāṃ vastra-garbhābhyāṃ manye gāḍhaṃ nipīḍayet ।।

anye gāḍhaṃ prapīḍayet
danta-prapīḍanotkāsa-gaṇḍādhmānāni cācaret ।
pṛṣṭhato yantrayec cainaṃ vastram āveṣṭayan naraḥ ।।

astram āveṣṭayen naraḥ
kandharāyāṃ parikṣipya nyasyāntar vāma-tarjanīm ।
eṣo antar-mukha-varjyānāṃ sirāṇāṃ yantraṇe vidhiḥ ।।

asyāntar vāma-tarjanīm ṣo antar-mukha-varjānāṃ
tato madhyamayāṅgulyā vaidyo aṅguṣṭha-vimuktayā ।
tāḍayed utthitāṃ jñātvā sparśād vāṅguṣṭha-pīḍanaiḥ ।।

parśāṅguṣṭha-prapīḍanaiḥ
kuṭhāryā lakṣayen madhye vāma-hasta-gṛhītayā ।
phaloddeśe su-niṣ-kampaṃ sirāṃ tad-vac ca mokṣayet ।।

tāḍayan pīḍayaṃś caināṃ vidhyed vrīhi-mukhena tu ।
aṅguṣṭhenonnamayyāgre nāsikām upa-nāsikām ।।

āḍayan pīḍayan vaināṃ āḍayan pīḍayec caināṃ
abhyunnata-vidaṣṭāgra-jihvasyādhas tad-āśrayām ।
yantrayet stanayor ūrdhvaṃ grīvāśrita-sirā-vyadhe ।।

pāṣāṇa-garbha-hastasya jānu-sthe prasṛte bhuje ।
kukṣer ārabhya mṛdite vidhyed baddhordhva-paṭṭake ।।

vidhyed dhasta-sirāṃ bāhāv an-ākuñcita-kūrpare ।
baddhvā sukhopaviṣṭasya muṣṭim aṅguṣṭha-garbhiṇam ।।

uṣṭim aṅguṣṭha-garbhiṇīm
ūrdhvaṃ vedhya-pradeśāc ca paṭṭikāṃ catur-aṅgule ।
vidhyed ālambamānasya bāhubhyāṃ pārśvayoḥ sirām ।।

prahṛṣṭe mehane jaṅghā-sirāṃ jānuny a-kuñcite ।
pāde tu su-sthite adhas-tāj jānu-saṃdher nipīḍite ।।

āde tu bhū-sthite adhas-tāj
gāḍhaṃ karābhyām ā-gulphaṃ caraṇe tasya copari ।
dvitīye kuñcite kiñ-cid-ārūḍhe hasta-vat tataḥ ।।

baddhvā vidhyet sirām ittham an-ukteṣv api kalpayet ।
teṣu teṣu pradeśeṣu tat tad yantram upāya-vit ।।

māṃsale nikṣiped deśe vrīhy-āsyaṃ vrīhi-mātrakam ।
yavārdham asthnām upari sirāṃ vidhyan kuṭhārikām ।।

irāṃ vidhyan kuṭhārayā irāṃ vidhyet kuṭhārayā 
sirāṃ vidhyet kuṭhārikām
samyag-viddhā sraved dhārāṃ yantre mukte tu na sravet ।
alpa-kālaṃ vahaty alpaṃ dur-viddhā taila-cūrṇanaiḥ ।।

amyag-viddhe sraved dhārā antre mukte ca na sravet 
ur-viddhā taila-cūrṇitaiḥ
sa-śabdam ati-viddhā tu sraved duḥkhena dhāryate ।
bhī-mūrchā-yantra-śaithilya-kuṇṭha-śastrāti-tṛptayaḥ ।।

kṣāma-tva-vegi-tā-svedā raktasyā-sruti-hetavaḥ ।
a-samyag asre sravati vella-vyoṣa-niśā-nataiḥ ।।

sāgāra-dhūma-lavaṇa-tailair dihyāt sirā-mukham ।
samyak-pravṛtte koṣṇena tailena lavaṇena ca ।।

ailena lavaṇena vā
agre sravati duṣṭāsraṃ kusumbhād iva pītikā ।
samyak srutvā svayaṃ tiṣṭhec chuddhaṃ tad iti nāharet ।।

yantraṃ vimucya mūrchāyāṃ vījite vyajanaiḥ punaḥ ।
srāvayen mūrchati punas tv apare-dyus try-ahe api vā ।।

vātāc chyāvāruṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ vega-srāvy accha-phenilaṃ ।
pittāt pītāsitaṃ visram a-skandy auṣṇyāt sa-candrikam ।।

-skandy auṣṇyāt sa-candrakam
vātikaṃ śoṇitaṃ śīghraṃ bhūmiḥ pibati cāvṛtam ।
makṣikāṇām a-kāntaṃ ca raktaṃ bhavati paittikam ।।
ślaiṣmikaṃ makṣikākrāntaṃ śuṣyaty api na ceṇayat ।।
kaphāt snigdham asṛk pāṇḍu tantu-mat picchilaṃ ghanam ।
saṃsṛṣṭa-liṅgaṃ saṃsargāt tri-doṣaṃ malināvilam ।।

a-śuddhau balino apy asraṃ na prasthāt srāvayet param ।
ati-srutau hi mṛtyuḥ syād dāruṇā vā calāmayāḥ ।।

-śuddhaṃ balino apy asraṃ
tatrābhyaṅga-rasa-kṣīra-rakta-pānāni bheṣajam ।
srute rakte śanair yantram apanīya himāmbunā ।।

prakṣālya taila-plotāktaṃ bandhanīyaṃ sirā-mukham ।
a-śuddhaṃ srāvayed bhūyaḥ sāyam ahny apare api vā ।।

-śuddhau srāvayed bhūyaḥ
snehopaskṛta-dehasya pakṣād vā bhṛśa-dūṣitam ।
kiñ-cid dhi śeṣe duṣṭāsre naiva rogo ativartate ।।

sa-śeṣam apy ato dhāryaṃ na cāti-srutim ācaret ।
harec chṛṅgādibhiḥ śeṣaṃ prasādam atha-vā nayet ।।

śītopacāra-pittāsra-kriyā-śuddhi-viśoṣaṇaiḥ ।
duṣṭaṃ raktam an-udriktam evam eva prasādayet ।।

rakte tv a-tiṣṭhati kṣipraṃ stambhanīm ācaret kriyām ।
lodhra-priyaṅgu-pattaṅga-māṣa-yaṣṭy-āhva-gairikaiḥ ।।

mṛt-kapālāñjana-kṣauma-maṣī-kṣīri-tvag-aṅkuraiḥ ।
vicūrṇayed vraṇa-mukhaṃ padmakādi-himaṃ pibet ।।

tām eva vā sirāṃ vidhyed vyadhāt tasmād an-antaram ।
sirā-mukhaṃ vā tvaritaṃ dahet tapta-śalākayā ।।

irā-mukhaṃ ca tvaritaṃ
un-mārga-gā yantra-nipīḍanena sva-sthānam āyānti punar na yāvat ।
doṣāḥ praduṣṭā rudhiraṃ prapannās tāvad dhitāhāra-vihāra-bhāk syāt ।।

nāty-uṣṇa-śītaṃ laghu dīpanīyaṃ rakte apanīte hitam anna-pānam ।
tadā śarīraṃ hy an-avasthitāsṛg agnir viśeṣād iti rakṣitavyaḥ ।।

adā śarīraṃ hy an-avasthitāsram gnir viśeṣād iti rakṣaṇīyaḥ 
gnir viśeṣeṇa ca rakṣitavyaḥ
prasanna-varṇendriyam indriyārthān icchantam a-vyāhata-paktṛ-vegam ।
sukhānvitaṃ puṣṭi-balopapannaṃ viśuddha-raktaṃ puruṣaṃ vadanti ।।

rakta-jā vyaṅga-kuṣṭhādyāḥ kaṇṭhāsyākṣi-śiro-gadāḥ ।
palitārūṃṣikābādhāḥ śāmyanty ete sirā-vyadhāt ।।

nir-vyādhi-nīlotpala-pattra-netraṃ su-vyakta-mūlāsita-baddha-keśam ।
candropamaṃ padma-su-gandhi vaktraṃ bhavel lalāṭe tu sirā-vyadhena ।।

sūtrasthāna
vakrarju-tiryag-ūrdhvādhaḥ śalyānāṃ pañca-dhā gatiḥ ।
dhyāmaṃ śopha-rujā-vantaṃ sravantaṃ śoṇitaṃ muhuḥ ।।

abhyudgataṃ budbuda-vat piṭikopacitaṃ vraṇam ।
mṛdu-māṃsaṃ ca jānīyād antaḥ-śalyaṃ samāsataḥ ।।

bhyunnataṃ budbuda-vat ṛdu-māṃsaṃ vijānīyād
viśeṣāt tvag-gate śalye vi-varṇaḥ kaṭhināyataḥ ।
śopho bhavati māṃsa-sthe coṣaḥ śopho vivardhate ।।

pīḍanā-kṣama-tā pākaḥ śalya-mārgo na rohati ।
peśy-antara-gate māṃsa-prāpta-vac chvayathuṃ vinā ।।

īḍane a-kṣama-tā pākaḥ -prāpta-vac chvayathor vinā
ākṣepaḥ snāyu-jālasya saṃrambha-stambha-vedanāḥ ।
snāyu-ge dur-haraṃ caitat sirādhmānaṃ sirāśrite ।।

nāva-ge dur-haraṃ caitat
sva-karma-guṇa-hāniḥ syāt srotasāṃ srotasi sthite ।
dhamanī-sthe anile raktaṃ phena-yuktam udīrayet ।।

hena-yuktam udīrayan
niryāti śabda-vān syāc ca hṛl-lāsaḥ sāṅga-vedanaḥ ।
saṃgharṣo bala-vān asthi-saṃdhi-prāpte asthi-pūrṇa-tā ।।

aṃharṣo bala-vān asthi-
naika-rūpā rujo asthi-sthe śophas tad-vac ca saṃdhi-ge ।
ceṣṭā-nivṛttiś ca bhaved āṭopaḥ koṣṭha-saṃśrite ।।

ānāho anna-śakṛn-mūtra-darśanaṃ ca vraṇānane ।
vidyān marma-gataṃ śalyaṃ marma-viddhopalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

yathā-svaṃ ca parisrāvais tvag-ādiṣu vibhāvayet ।
ruhyate śuddha-dehānām anuloma-sthitaṃ tu tat ।।

athā-yathaṃ parisrāvais
doṣa-kopābhighātādi-kṣobhād bhūyo api bādhate ।
tvaṅ-naṣṭe yatra tatra syur abhyaṅga-sveda-mardanaiḥ ।।

rāga-rug-dāha-saṃrambhā yatra cājyaṃ vilīyate ।
āśu śuṣyati lepo vā tat-sthānaṃ śalya-vad vadet ।।

atra vājyaṃ vilīyate āśuṣyati pralepo vā
māṃsa-praṇaṣṭaṃ saṃśuddhyā karśanāc chlatha-tāṃ gatam ।
kṣobhād rāgādibhiḥ śalyaṃ lakṣayet tad-vad eva ca ।।

arṣaṇāc chlatha-tāṃ gatam
peśy-asthi-saṃdhi-koṣṭheṣu naṣṭam asthiṣu lakṣayet ।
asthnām abhyañjana-sveda-bandha-pīḍana-mardanaiḥ ।।

prasāraṇākuñcanataḥ saṃdhi-naṣṭaṃ tathāsthi-vat ।
naṣṭe snāyu-sirā-sroto-dhamanīṣv a-same pathi ।।

aśva-yuktaṃ rathaṃ khaṇḍa-cakram āropya rogiṇam ।
śīghraṃ nayet tatas tasya saṃrambhāc chalyam ādiśet ।।

marma-naṣṭaṃ pṛthaṅ noktaṃ teṣāṃ māṃsādi-saṃśrayāt ।
sāmānyena sa-śalyaṃ tu kṣobhiṇyā kriyayā sa-ruk ।।

vṛttaṃ pṛthu catuṣ-koṇaṃ tri-puṭaṃ ca samāsataḥ ।
a-dṛśya-śalya-saṃsthānaṃ vraṇākṛtyā vibhāvayet ।।

teṣām āharaṇopāyau pratilomānulomakau ।
arvācīna-parācīne nirharet tad-viparyayāt ।।

vācīna-parācīne
sukhāhāryaṃ yataś chittvā tatas tiryag-gataṃ haret ।
śalyaṃ na nirghātyam uraḥ-kakṣā-vaṅkṣaṇa-pārśva-gam ।।

pratilomam an-uttuṇḍaṃ chedyaṃ pṛthu-mukhaṃ ca yat ।
naivāhared vi-śalya-ghnaṃ naṣṭaṃ vā nir-upadravam ।।

athāharet kara-prāpyaṃ kareṇaivetarat punaḥ ।
dṛśyaṃ siṃhāhi-makara-varmi-karkaṭakānanaiḥ ।।

a-dṛśyaṃ vraṇa-saṃsthānād grahītuṃ śakyate yataḥ ।
kaṅka-bhṛṅgāhva-kurara-śarāri-vāyasānanaiḥ ।।

saṃdaṃśābhyāṃ tvag-ādi-sthaṃ tālābhyāṃ suṣiraṃ haret ।
suṣira-sthaṃ tu nalakaiḥ śeṣaṃ śeṣair yathā-yatham ।।

śastreṇa vā viśasyādau tato nir-lohitaṃ vraṇam ।
kṛtvā ghṛtena saṃsvedya baddhācārikam ādiśet ।।

addhācārikam ācaret
sirā-snāyu-vilagnaṃ tu cālayitvā śalākayā ।
hṛdaye saṃsthitaṃ śalyaṃ trāsitasya himāmbunā ।।

irā-snāyu-vilagnaṃ ca irā-snāva-vilagnaṃ tu
tataḥ sthānāntaraṃ prāptaṃ āharet tad yathā-yatham ।
yathā-mārgaṃ dur-ākarṣam anyato apy evam āharet ।।

asthi-daṣṭe naraṃ padbhyāṃ pīḍayitvā vinirharet ।
ity a-śakye su-balibhiḥ su-gṛhītasya kiṅkaraiḥ ।।

sthi-dṛṣṭe naraṃ padbhyāṃ sthi-naṣṭe naraṃ padbhyāṃ 
sthi-lagnaṃ naraṃ padbhyāṃ sthi-sthaṃ na paraṃ padbhyāṃ
tathāpy a-śakye vāraṅgaṃ vakrī-kṛtya dhanur-jyayā ।
su-baddhaṃ vaktra-kaṭake badhnīyāt su-samāhitaḥ ।।

su-saṃyatasya pañcāṅgyā vājinaḥ kaśayātha tam ।
tāḍayed iti mūrdhānaṃ vegenonnamayan yathā ।।

egenonnamayed yathā
uddharec chalyam evaṃ vā śākhāyāṃ kalpayet taroḥ ।
baddhvā dur-bala-vāraṅgaṃ kuśābhiḥ śalyam āharet ।।

śvayathu-grasta-vāraṅgaṃ śopham utpīḍya yuktitaḥ ।
mudgarāhatayā nāḍyā nirghātyottuṇḍitaṃ haret ।।

tair eva cānayen mārgam a-mārgottuṇḍitaṃ tu yat ।
mṛditvā karṇināṃ karṇaṃ nāḍy-āsyena nigṛhya vā ।।

enaiva vā nayen mārgam -mārgottuṇḍitaṃ ca yat
ayas-kāntena niṣ-karṇaṃ vivṛtāsyam ṛju-sthitam ।
pakvāśaya-gataṃ śalyaṃ virekeṇa vinirharet ।।

duṣṭa-vāta-viṣa-stanya-rakta-toyādi cūṣaṇaiḥ ।
kaṇṭha-sroto-gate śalye sūtraṃ kaṇṭhe praveśayet ।।

bisenātte tataḥ śalye bisaṃ sūtraṃ samaṃ haret ।
nāḍyāgni-tāpitāṃ kṣiptvā śalākām ap-sthirī-kṛtām ।।

atu-digdham a-jātuṣam
ānayej jātuṣaṃ kaṇṭhāj jatu-digdhām a-jātuṣam ।
keśondukena pītena dravaiḥ kaṇṭakam ākṣipet ।।

atu-digdham a-jātuṣam eśāṇḍakena pītena eśāṇḍukena pītena 
eśoṇḍukena pītena
sahasā sūtra-baddhena vamatas tena cetarat ।
a-śakyaṃ mukha-nāsābhyām āhartuṃ parato nudet ।।

ap-pāna-skandha-ghātābhyāṃ grāsa-śalyaṃ praveśayet ।
sūkṣmākṣi-vraṇa-śalyāni kṣauma-vāla-jalair haret ।।

apāṃ pūrṇaṃ vidhunuyād avāk-śirasam āyatam ।
vāmayec cā-mukhaṃ bhasma-rāśau vā nikhanen naram ।।

āmayed ā-mukhaṃ bhasma- āmayed vā-mukhaṃ bhasma- 
āmayed vā sukhaṃ bhasma-
karṇe ambu-pūrṇe hastena mathitvā taila-vāriṇī ।
kṣiped adho-mukhaṃ karṇaṃ hanyād vācūṣayeta vā ।।

anyād vācūṣayet tadā anyād vācūṣayeta ca
kīṭe sroto-gate karṇaṃ pūrayed lavaṇāmbunā ।
śuktena vā sukhoṣṇena mṛte kleda-haro vidhiḥ ।।

jātuṣaṃ hema-rūpyādi-dhātu-jaṃ ca cira-sthitam ।
ūṣmaṇā prāya-śaḥ śalyaṃ deha-jena vilīyate ।।

mṛd-veṇu-dāru-śṛṅgāsthi-danta-vālopalāni na ।
viṣāṇa-veṇv-ayas-tāla-dāru-śalyaṃ cirād api ।।

-danta-vālopalādi na
prāyo nirbhujyate tad dhi pacaty āśu palāsṛjī ।
śalye māṃsāvagāḍhe cet sa deśo na vidahyate ।।

śalye māṃsāvagāḍhe ca
tatas taṃ mardana-sveda-śuddhi-karṣaṇa-bṛṃhaṇaiḥ ।
tīkṣṇopanāha-pānānna-ghana-śastra-padāṅkanaiḥ ।।

-śuddhi-karśana-bṛṃhaṇaiḥ
pācayitvā harec chalyaṃ pāṭanaiṣaṇa-bhedanaiḥ ।
śalya-pradeśa-yantrāṇām avekṣya bahu-rūpa-tām ।।
tais tair upāyair mati-mān śalyaṃ vidyāt tathāharet ।।
ū̆śalyaṃ vidyāt tato haret

sūtrasthāna
vraṇaḥ saṃjāyate prāyaḥ pākāc chvayathu-pūrvakāt ।
tam evopacaret tasmād rakṣan pākaṃ prayatnataḥ ।।

su-śīta-lepa-sekāsra-mokṣa-saṃśodhanādibhiḥ ।
śopho alpo alpoṣma-ruk sāmaḥ sa-varṇaḥ kaṭhinaḥ sthiraḥ ।।

u-śīta-lepa-sekāsṛṅ- śopho alpo alpoṣma-ruk cāmaḥ
pacyamāno vi-varṇas tu rāgī vastir ivātataḥ ।
sphuṭatīva sa-nistodaḥ sāṅga-marda-vijṛmbhikaḥ ।।

saṃrambhā-ruci-dāhoṣā-tṛḍ-jvarā-nidra-tānvitaḥ ।
styānaṃ viṣyandayaty ājyaṃ vraṇa-vat sparśanā-sahaḥ ।।

pakve alpa-vega-tā mlāniḥ pāṇḍu-tā vali-saṃbhavaḥ ।
nāmo anteṣūnnatir madhye kaṇḍū-śophādi-mārdavam ।।

akve alpa-vega-tā glāniḥ akve alpa-vedanā glāniḥ akve alpa-vedanā mlāniḥ 
akve alpā vedanā mlāniḥ
spṛṣṭe pūyasya saṃcāro bhaved vastāv ivāmbhasaḥ ।
śūlaṃ narte anilād dāhaḥ pittāc chophaḥ kaphodayāt ।।

rāgo raktāc ca pākaḥ syād ato doṣaiḥ sa-śoṇitaiḥ ।
pāke ativṛtte suṣiras tanu-tvag-doṣa-bhakṣitaḥ ।।

valībhir ācitaḥ śyāvaḥ śīryamāṇa-tanū-ruhaḥ ।
kapha-jeṣu tu śopheṣu gambhīraṃ pākam ety asṛk ।।

alībhir ācitaḥ śyāmaḥ
pakva-liṅgaṃ tato a-spaṣṭaṃ yatra syāc chīta-śopha-tā ।
tvak-sāvarṇyaṃ rujo alpa-tvaṃ ghana-sparśa-tvam aśma-vat ।।

rakta-pākam iti brūyāt taṃ prājño mukta-saṃśayaḥ ।
alpa-sat-tve a-bale bāle pākād vāty-artham uddhate ।।

ākād aty-artham uddhate āke vāty-artham uddhate
dāraṇaṃ marma-saṃdhy-ādi-sthite cānya-tra pāṭanam ।
āma-cchede sirā-snāyu-vyāpado asṛg-ati-srutiḥ ।।

rujo ati-vṛddhir daraṇaṃ visarpo vā kṣatodbhavaḥ ।
tiṣṭhann antaḥ punaḥ pūyaḥ sirā-snāyv-asṛg-āmiṣam ।।

vivṛddho dahati kṣipraṃ tṛṇolapam ivānalaḥ ।
yaś chinatty āmam a-jñānād yaś ca pakvam upekṣate ।।

ṛṇolupam ivānalaḥ ṛṇopalam ivānalaḥ ṛṇoccayam 
ivānalaḥ
śva-pacāv iva vijñeyau tāv a-niścita-kāriṇau ।
prāk śastra-karmaṇaś ceṣṭaṃ bhojayed annam āturam ।।

śva-pacāv iva jānīyāt vāv a-niścita-kāriṇau rāk 
śastra-karmaṇaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ
pāna-paṃ pāyayen madyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ yo vedanā-kṣamaḥ ।
na mūrchaty anna-saṃyogān mattaḥ śastraṃ na budhyate ।।

anya-tra mūḍha-garbhāśma-mukha-rogodarāturāt ।
athāhṛtopakaraṇaṃ vaidyaḥ prāṅ-mukham āturam ।।

thāhṛtopakaraṇo
saṃmukho yantrayitvāśu nyasyen marmādi varjayan ।
anulomaṃ su-niśitaṃ śastram ā-pūya-darśanāt ।।

aṃmukhaṃ yantrayitvāśu
sakṛd evāharec tac ca pāke tu su-mahaty api ।
pāṭayed dvy-aṅgulaṃ samyag dvy-aṅgula-try-aṅgulāntaram ।।

eṣitvā samyag eṣiṇyā paritaḥ su-nirūpitam ।
aṅgulī-nāla-vālair vā yathā-deśaṃ yathāśayam ।।

yato gatāṃ gatiṃ vidyād utsaṅgo yatra yatra ca ।
tatra tatra vraṇaṃ kuryāt su-vibhaktaṃ nir-āśayam ।।

tsaṅgaṃ yatra yatra ca
āyataṃ ca viśālaṃ ca yathā doṣo na tiṣṭhati ।
śauryam āśu-kriyā tīkṣṇaṃ śastram a-sveda-vepathū ।।

śauryam āśu-kriyā tīkṣṇa- -śastram a-sveda-vepathū
a-saṃmohaś ca vaidyasya śastra-karmaṇi śasyate ।
tiryak chindyāl lalāṭa-bhrū-danta-veṣṭaka-jatruṇi ।।

kukṣi-kakṣākṣi-kūṭauṣṭha-kapola-gala-vaṅkṣaṇe ।
anya-tra cchedanāt tiryak sirā-snāyu-vipāṭanam ।।

śastre avacārite vāgbhiḥ śītāmbhobhiś ca rogiṇam ।
āśvāsya parito aṅgulyā paripīḍya vraṇaṃ tataḥ ।।

kṣālayitvā kaṣāyeṇa plotenāmbho apanīya ca ।
guggulv-aguru-siddhārtha-hiṅgu-sarja-rasānvitaiḥ ।।

dhūpayec paṭu-ṣaḍgranthā-nimba-pattrair ghṛta-plutaiḥ ।
tila-kalkājya-madhubhir yathā-svaṃ bheṣajena ca ।।

digdhāṃ vartiṃ tato dadyāt tair evācchādayec ca tām ।
ghṛtāktaiḥ saktubhiś cordhvaṃ ghanāṃ kavalikāṃ tataḥ ।।

air evācchādayec ca tam
nidhāya yuktyā badhnīyāt paṭṭena su-samāhitam ।
pārśve savye apa-savye vā nādhas-tān naiva copari ।।

aṭṭena su-samāhitaḥ
śuci-sūkṣma-dṛḍhāḥ paṭṭāḥ kavalyaḥ sa-vikeśikāḥ ।
dhūpitā mṛdavaḥ ślakṣṇā nir-valīkā vraṇe hitāḥ ।।

avalyaḥ su-vikeśikāḥ
kurvītān-antaraṃ tasya rakṣāṃ rakṣo-niṣiddhaye ।
baliṃ copaharet tebhyaḥ sadā mūrdhnā ca dhārayet ।।

urvītān-antaraṃ samyag- akṣāṃ rakṣo-nivṛttaye 
-rakṣāṃ rakṣo-niṣiddhaye adā mūrdhnāvadhārayet
lakṣmīṃ guhām atiguhāṃ jaṭilāṃ brahmacāriṇīm ।
vacāṃ chattrām aticchattrāṃ dūrvāṃ siddhārthakān api ।।

tataḥ sneha-dinehoktaṃ tasyācāraṃ samādiśet ।
divā-svapno vraṇe kaṇḍū-rāga-ruk-śopha-pūya-kṛt ।।

ataḥ sneha-vidhānoktaṃ
strīṇāṃ tu smṛti-saṃsparśa-darśanaiś calita-srute ।
śukre vyavāya-jān doṣān a-saṃsarge apy avāpnuyāt ।।

vraṇe śvayathur āyāsāt sa ca rāgaś ca jāgarāt ।
tau ca ruk ca divā-svāpāt tāś ca mṛtyuś ca maithunāt ।।

bhojanaṃ ca yathā-sātmyaṃ yava-godhūma-ṣaṣṭikāḥ ।
masūra-mudga-tubarī-jīvantī-suniṣaṇṇakāḥ ।।

hojanaṃ tu yathā-sātmyaṃ
bāla-mūlaka-vārtāka-taṇḍulīyaka-vāstukam ।
kāravellaka-karkoṭa-paṭola-kaṭukā-phalam ।।

saindhavaṃ dāḍimaṃ dhātrī ghṛtaṃ tapta-himaṃ jalam ।
jīrṇa-śāly-odanaṃ snigdham alpam uṣṇodakottaram ।।

lpam uṣṇaṃ dravottaram
bhuñjāno jāṅgalair māṃsaiḥ śīghraṃ vraṇam apohati ।
aśitaṃ mātrayā kāle pathyaṃ yāti jarāṃ sukham ।।

a-jīrṇāt tv anilādīnāṃ vibhramo bala-vān bhavet ।
tataḥ śopha-rujā-pāka-dāhānāhān avāpnuyāt ।।

-jīrṇe tv anilādīnāṃ
navaṃ dhānyaṃ tilān māṣān madyaṃ māṃsam a-jāṅgalam ।
kṣīrekṣu-vikṛtīr amlaṃ lavaṇaṃ kaṭukaṃ tyajet ।।

adyaṃ māṃsaṃ tv a-jāṅgalam
yac cānyad api viṣṭambhi vidāhi guru śītalam ।
vargo ayaṃ nava-dhānyādir vraṇinaḥ sarva-doṣa-kṛt ।।

raṇināṃ sarva-doṣa-kṛt
madyaṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇa-rūkṣāmlam āśu vyāpādayed vraṇam ।
vālośīraiś ca vījyeta na cainaṃ parighaṭṭayet ।।

ālośīraiś ca vījyeta
na tuden na ca kaṇḍūyec ceṣṭamānaś ca pālayet ।
snigdha-vṛddha-dvi-jātīnāṃ kathāḥ śṛṇvan manaḥ-priyāḥ ।।

hayānaḥ paripālayet iddha-vṛddha-dvi-jātīnāṃ
āśā-vān vyādhi-mokṣāya kṣipraṃ vraṇam apohati ।
tṛtīye ahni punaḥ kuryād vraṇa-karma ca pūrva-vat ।।

prakṣālanādi divase dvitīye nācaret tathā ।
tīvra-vyatho vigrathitaś cirāt saṃrohati vraṇaḥ ।।

snigdhāṃ rūkṣāṃ ślathāṃ gāḍhāṃ dur-nyastāṃ ca vikeśikām ।
vraṇe na dadyāt kalkaṃ vā snehāt kledo vivardhate ।।

māṃsa-cchedo ati-rug-raukṣyād daraṇaṃ śoṇitāgamaḥ ।
ślathāti-gāḍha-dur-nyāsair vraṇa-vartmāvagharṣaṇam ।।

ślathāti-gāḍha-dur-nyastair
sa-pūti-māṃsaṃ sotsaṅgaṃ sa-gatiṃ pūya-garbhiṇam ।
vraṇaṃ viśodhayec chīghraṃ sthitā hy antar vikeśikā ।।

vy-amlaṃ tu pāṭitaṃ śophaṃ pācanaiḥ samupācaret ।
bhojanair upanāhaiś ca nāti-vraṇa-virodhibhiḥ ।।

āti-vraṇa-viśodhibhiḥ
sadyaḥ sadyo-vraṇān sīvyed vivṛtān abhighāta-jān ।
medo-jāō̃ likhitān granthīn hrasvāḥ pālīś ca karṇayoḥ ।।

śiro-'kṣi-kūṭa-nāsauṣṭha-gaṇḍa-karṇoru-bāhuṣu ।
grīvā-lalāṭa-muṣka-sphiṅ-meḍhra-pāyūdarādiṣu ।।

gambhīreṣu pradeśeṣu māṃsaleṣv a-caleṣu ca ।
na tu vaṅkṣaṇa-kakṣādāv alpa-māṃse cale vraṇān ।।

lpa-māṃsa-cale vraṇān lpa-māṃsa-calān vraṇān
vāyu-nirvāhiṇaḥ śalya-garbhān kṣāra-viṣāgni-jān ।
sīvyec calāsthi-śuṣkāsra-tṛṇa-romāpanīya tu ।।

-tṛṇa-romāpanīya ca
pralambi māṃsaṃ vicchinnaṃ niveśya sva-niveśane ।
saṃdhy-asthi ca sthite rakte snāyvā sūtreṇa valkalaiḥ ।।

aṃdhy-asthy avasthite rakte nāvnā sūtreṇa valkalaiḥ
sīvyen na dūre nāsanne gṛhṇan nālpaṃ na vā bahu ।
sāntvayitvā tataś cārtaṃ vraṇe madhu-ghṛta-drutaiḥ ।।

raṇe madhu-ghṛta-plutaiḥ añjana-kṣauma-ja-maṣī-phalinī-śallakī-phalaiḥ । 
ṛhṇan sv-alpaṃ na vā bahu śāntayitvā tataś cārtaṃ v
sāntayitvā tataś cārtaṃ
sa-lodhra-madhukair digdhe yuñjyād bandhādi pūrva-vat ।।

vraṇo niḥ-śoṇitauṣṭho yaḥ kiñ-cid evāvalikhya tam ।
saṃjāta-rudhiraṃ sīvyet saṃdhānaṃ hy asya śoṇitam ।।

bandhanāni tu deśādīn vīkṣya yuñjīta teṣu ca ।
iñ-cid eva vilikhya tam
āvikājina-kauśeyam uṣṇaṃ kṣaumaṃ tu śītalam ।।

śītoṣṇaṃ tulā-saṃtāna-kārpāsa-snāyu-valka-jam ।
tāmrāyas-trapu-sīsāni vraṇe medaḥ-kaphādhike ।।

-kārpāsa-snāva-valka-jam
bhaṅge ca yuñjyāt phalakaṃ carma-valka-kuśādi ca ।
sva-nāmānugatākārā bandhās tu daśa pañca ca ।।

kośa-svastika-muttolī-cīna-dāmānuvellitam ।
khaṭvā-vibandha-sthagikā-vitānotsaṅga-goṣ-phaṇāḥ ।।

-vitānotsaṅga-go-phaṇāḥ
yamakaṃ maṇḍalākhyaṃ ca pañcāṅgī ceti yojayet ।
yo yatra su-niviṣṭaḥ syāt taṃ teṣāṃ tatra buddhi-mān ।।

o yatra saṃniviṣṭaḥ syāt
vidadhyāt teṣu teṣv eva kośam aṅguli-parvasu ।
svastikaṃ karṇa-kakṣādi-staneṣūktaṃ ca saṃdhiṣu ।।

muttolīṃ meḍhra-grīvādau yuñjyāc cīnam apāṅgayoḥ ।
saṃbādhe aṅge tathā dāma śākhāsv evānuvellitam ।।

khaṭvāṃ gaṇḍe hanau śaṅkhe vibandhaṃ pṛṣṭhakodare ।
aṅguṣṭhāṅgulimeḍhrāgre sthagikām antra-vṛddhiṣu ।।

vitānaṃ pṛthulāṅgādau tathā śirasi cerayet ।
vilambini tathotsaṅgaṃ nāsauṣṭha-cibukādiṣu ।।

goṣ-phaṇaṃ saṃdhiṣu tathā yamakaṃ yamike vraṇe ।
vṛtte aṅge maṇḍalākhyaṃ ca pañcāṅgīṃ cordhva-jatruṣu ।।

badhnīyād gāḍham ūru-sphik-kakṣā-vaṅkṣaṇa-mūrdhasu ।
śākhā-vadana-karṇoraḥ-pṛṣṭha-pārśva-galodare ।।

samaṃ mehana-muṣke ca netre saṃdhiṣu ca ślatham ।
badhnīyāc chithila-sthāne vāta-śleṣmodbhave samam ।।

gāḍham eva sama-sthāne bhṛśaṃ gāḍhaṃ tad-āśaye ।
śīte vasante api ca tau mokṣaṇīyau try-ahāt try-ahāt ।।

hṛśaṃ gāḍhaṃ tad-āśraye śīte vasante ca tathā 
okṣayet tau try-ahāt try-ahāt okṣaṇīyas try-ahāt try-ahāt
pitta-raktotthayor bandho gāḍha-sthāne samo mataḥ ।
sama-sthāne ślatho naiva śithilasyāśaye tathā ।।

sāyaṃ prātas tayor mokṣo grīṣme śaradi ceṣyate ।
a-baddho daṃśa-maśaka-śīta-vātādi-pīḍitaḥ ।।

duṣṭī-bhavec ciraṃ cātra na tiṣṭhet sneha-bheṣajam ।
kṛcchreṇa śuddhiṃ rūḍhiṃ vā yāti rūḍho vi-varṇa-tām ।।

baddhas tu cūrṇito bhagno viśliṣṭaḥ pāṭito api vā ।
chinna-snāyu-siro apy āśu sukhaṃ saṃrohati vraṇaḥ ।।

utthāna-śayanādyāsu sarvehāsu na pīḍyate ।
udvṛttauṣṭhaḥ samutsanno viṣamaḥ kaṭhino ati-ruk ।।

arvehāsu na pīḍayet ddhṛtauṣṭhaḥ samutsanno
samo mṛdur a-ruk śīghraṃ vraṇaḥ śudhyati rohati ।
sthirāṇām alpa-māṃsānāṃ raukṣyād an-uparohatām ।।

pracchādyam auṣadhaṃ pattrair yathā-doṣaṃ yathartu ca ।
a-jīrṇa-taruṇāc chidraiḥ samantāt su-niveśitaiḥ ।।

-jīrṇā-taruṇāc chidraiḥ
dhautair a-karkaśaiḥ kṣīri-bhūrjārjuna-kadamba-jaiḥ ।
kuṣṭhinām agni-dagdhānāṃ piṭikā madhu-mehinām ।।

karṇikāś conduru-viṣe kṣāra-dagdhā viṣānvitāḥ ।
bandhanīyā na māṃs-pāke guda-pāke ca dāruṇe ।।

a māṃs-pāke ca badhnīyād āṃsa-pāke na badhnīyād
śīryamāṇāḥ sa-rug-dāhāḥ śophāvasthā-visarpiṇaḥ ।
a-rakṣayā vraṇe yasmin makṣikā nikṣipet kṛmīn ।।

te bhakṣayantaḥ kurvanti rujā-śophāsra-saṃsravān ।
surasādiṃ prayuñjīta tatra dhāvana-pūraṇe ।।

ujā-śophāsra-visrutīḥ
saptaparṇa-karañjārka-nimba-rājādana-tvacaḥ ।
go-mūtra-kalkito lepaḥ sekaḥ kṣārāmbunā hitaḥ ।।

o-mūtra-kalkitālepaḥ
pracchādya māṃsa-peśyā vā vraṇaṃ tān āśu nirharet ।
na cainaṃ tvaramāṇo antaḥ sa-doṣam uparohayet ।।

so alpenāpy apacāreṇa bhūyo vikurute yataḥ ।
rūḍhe apy a-jīrṇa-vyāyāma-vyavāyādīn vivarjayet ।।

harṣaṃ krodhaṃ bhayaṃ cāpi yāvad ā-sthairya-saṃbhavāt ।
ādareṇānuvartyo ayaṃ māsān ṣaṭ sapta vā vidhiḥ ।।

arṣaṃ krodhaṃ bhayaṃ vāpi
utpadyamānāsu ca tāsu tāsu vārtāsu doṣādi-balānusārī ।
tais tair upāyaiḥ prayataś cikitsed ālocayan vistaram uttaroktam ।।

sūtrasthāna
sarva-śastrānu-śastrāṇāṃ kṣāraḥ śreṣṭho bahūni yat ।
chedya-bhedyādi-karmāṇi kurute viṣameṣv api ।।

duḥkhāvacārya-śāstreṣu tena siddhim a-yātsu ca ।
ati-kṛcchreṣu rogeṣu yac ca pāne api yujyate ।।

ena siddhiṃ na yātsu ca
sa peyo arśo-'gni-sādāśma-gulmodara-garādiṣu ।
yojyaḥ sākṣān maṣa-śvitra-bāhyārśaḥ-kuṣṭha-suptiṣu ।।

bhagandarārbuda-granthi-duṣṭa-nāḍī-vraṇādiṣu ।
na tūbhayo api yoktavyaḥ pitte rakte cale a-bale ।।

hagandarāpacī-granthi- itte rakte bale a-bale
jvare atīsāre hṛn-mūrdha-roge pāṇḍv-āmaye a-rucau ।
timire kṛta-saṃśuddhau śvayathau sarva-gātra-ge ।।

śvayathau sarva-gātra-je
bhīru-garbhiṇy-ṛtu-matī-prodvṛtta-phala-yoniṣu ।
a-jīrṇe anne śiśau vṛddhe dhamanī-saṃdhi-marmasu ।।

taruṇāsthi-sirā-snāyu-sevanī-gala-nābhiṣu ।
deśe alpa-māṃse vṛṣaṇa-meḍhra-sroto-nakhāntare ।।

eśe alpa-māṃse vṛṣaṇe eḍhre sroto-nakhāntare
vartma-rogād ṛte akṣṇoś ca śīta-varṣoṣṇa-dur-dine ।
kāla-muṣkaka-śamyāka-kadalī-pāribhadrakān ।।

aśvakarṇa-mahāvṛkṣa-palāśāsphota-vṛkṣakān ।
indravṛkṣārka-pūtīka-naktamālāśvamārakān ।।

kākajaṅghām apāmārgam agnimanthāgni-tilvakān ।
sārdrān sa-mūla-śākhādīn khaṇḍa-śaḥ parikalpitān ।।

kośātakīs catasraś ca śūkaṃ nālaṃ yavasya ca ।
nivāte nicayī-kṛtya pṛthak tāni śilā-tale ।।

śūka-nālaṃ yavasya ca
prakṣipya muṣkaka-caye sudhāśmāni ca dīpayet ।
tatas tilānāṃ kutalair dagdhvāgnau vigate pṛthak ।।

atas tilānāṃ kutilair atas tilānāṃ kuntālair
kṛtvā sudhāśmanāṃ bhasma droṇaṃ tv itara-bhasmanaḥ ।
muṣkakottaram ādāya praty-ekaṃ jala-mūtrayoḥ ।।

roṇaṃ cetara-bhasmanaḥ
gālayed ardha-bhāreṇa mahatā vāsasā ca tat ।
yāvat picchila-raktācchas tīkṣṇo jātas tadā ca tam ।।

gṛhītvā kṣāra-niṣyandaṃ pacel lauhyāṃ vighaṭṭayan ।
pacyamāne tatas tasmiṃs tāḥ sudhā-bhasma-śarkarāḥ ।।

śuktīḥ kṣīra-pakaṃ śaṅkha-nābhīś cāyasa-bhājane ।
kṛtvāgni-varṇān bahu-śaḥ kṣārotthe kuḍavonmite ।।

ṃnābhīṃś cāyasa-bhājane ṣārācche kuḍavonmite
nirvāpya piṣṭvā tenaiva pratīvāpaṃ vinikṣipet ।
ślakṣṇaṃ śakṛd dakṣa-śikhi-gṛdhra-kaṅka-kapota-jam ।।

catuṣ-pāt-pakṣi-pittāla-manohvā-lavaṇāni ca ।
paritaḥ su-tarāṃ cāto darvyā tam avaghaṭtayet ।।

sa-bāṣpaiś ca yadottiṣṭhed budbudair leha-vad ghanaḥ ।
avatārya tadā śīto yava-rāśāv ayo-maye ।।

a-bāṣpaiś ca yadā tiṣṭhed vatārya tataḥ śīte vatārya tataḥ śīto vatārya tadā 
śīte
sthāpyo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ kṣāro na tu piṣṭvā kṣipen mṛdau ।
nirvāpyāpanayet tīkṣṇe pūrva-vat prativāpanam ।।

tathā lāṅgalikā-dantī-citrakātiviṣā-vacāḥ ।
svarjikā-kanakakṣīrī-hiṅgu-pūtika-pallavāḥ ।।

tālapattrī viḍaṃ ceti sapta-rātrāt paraṃ tu saḥ ।
yojyas tīkṣṇo anila-śleṣma-medo-jeṣv arbudādiṣu ।।

ālapattrī viḍaṅgaṃ ca
madhyeṣv eṣv eva madhyo anyaḥ pittāsra-guda-janmasu ।
balārthaṃ kṣīṇa-pānīye kṣārāmbu punar āvapet ।।

adhyeṣv eva ca madhyo anyaḥ adhyeṣv eṣu ca madhyo anyaḥ 
ittāsṛg-guda-janmasu
nāti-tīkṣṇa-mṛduḥ ślakṣṇaḥ picchilaḥ śīghra-gaḥ sitaḥ ।
śikharī sukha-nirvāpyo na viṣyandī na cāti-ruk ।।

āti-tīkṣṇo mṛduḥ ślakṣṇaḥ
kṣāro daśa-guṇaḥ śastra-tejasor api karma-kṛt ।
ācūṣann iva saṃrambhād gātram āpīḍayann iva ।।

sarvato anusaran doṣān unmūlayati mūlataḥ ।
karma kṛtvā gata-rujaḥ svayaṃ evopaśāmyati ।।

kṣāra-sādhye gade chinne likhite srāvite atha-vā ।
kṣāraṃ śalākayā dattvā plota-prāvṛta-dehayā ।।

lota-plāvita-dehayā
mātrā-śatam upekṣeta tatrārśaḥsv āvṛtānanam ।
hastena yantraṃ kurvīta vartma-rogeṣu vartmanī ।।

nirbhujya picunācchādya kṛṣṇa-bhāgaṃ vinikṣipet ।
padma-pattra-tanuḥ kṣāra-lepo ghrāṇārbudeṣu ca ।।

-lepo ghrāṇārbudeṣu tu
praty-ādityaṃ niṣaṇṇasya samunnamyāgra-nāsikām ।
mātrā vidhāryaḥ pañcāśat tad-vad arśasi karṇa-je ।।

amunnasyāgra-nāsikām ātrā vidhārya pañcāśat 
mātrā vidhāryāḥ pañcāśat
kṣāraṃ pramārjanenānu parimṛjyāvagamya ca ।
su-dagdhaṃ ghṛta-madhv-aktaṃ tat payo-mastu-kāñjikaiḥ ।।

ṣāraṃ pramārjanenāśu
nirvāpayet tataḥ sājyaiḥ svādu-śītaiḥ pradehayet ।
abhiṣyandīni bhojyāni bhojyāni kledanāya ca ।।

yadi ca sthira-mūla-tvāt kṣāra-dagdhaṃ na śīryate ।
dhānyāmla-bīja-yaṣṭy-āhva-tilair ālepayet tataḥ ।।

tila-kalkaḥ sa-madhuko ghṛtākto vraṇa-ropaṇaḥ ।
pakva-jambv-asitaṃ sannaṃ samyag-dagdhaṃ viparyaye ।।

akva-jambū-nibhaṃ sannaṃ
tāmra-tā-toda-kaṇḍv-ādyair dur-dagdhaṃ taṃ punar dahet ।
ati-dagdhe sraved raktaṃ mūrchā-dāha-jvarādayaḥ ।।

ur-dagdhaṃ tat punar dahet
gude viśeṣād viṇ-mūtra-saṃrodho ati-pravartanam ।
puṃs-tvopaghāto mṛtyur vā gudasya śātanād dhruvam ।।

udasya śātanaṃ dhruvam udasya sadanād dhruvam 
udasya sadanaṃ dhruvam
nāsāyāṃ nāsikā-vaṃśa-daraṇākuñcanodbhavaḥ ।
bhavec ca viṣayā-jñānaṃ tad-vac chrotrādikeṣv api ।।

viśeṣād atra seko amlair lepo madhu ghṛtaṃ tilāḥ ।
vāta-pitta-harā ceṣṭā sarvaiva śiśirā kriyā ।।

amlo hi śītaḥ sparśena kṣāras tenopasaṃhitaḥ ।
yāty āśu svādu-tāṃ tasmād amlair nirvāpayet-tarām ।।

viṣāgni-śastrāśani-mṛtyu-tulyaḥ kṣāro bhaved alpam ati-prayuktaḥ ।
rogān nihanyād a-cireṇa ghorān sa dhī-matā samyag-anuprayukto ।।

agniḥ kṣārād api śreṣṭhas tad-dagdhānām a-saṃbhavāt ।
bheṣaja-kṣāra-śastraiś ca na siddhānāṃ prasādhanāt ।।

tvaci māṃse sirā-snāyu-saṃdhy-asthiṣu sa yujyate ।
maṣāṅga-glāni-mūrdhārti-mantha-kīla-tilādiṣu ।।

-saṃdhy-asthiṣu sa yojyate
tvag-dāho varti-go-danta-sūrya-kānta-śarādibhiḥ ।
arśo-bhagandara-granthi-nāḍī-duṣṭa-vraṇādiṣu ।।

māṃsa-dāho madhu-sneha-jāmbavauṣṭha-guḍādibhiḥ ।
śliṣṭa-vartmany asṛk-srāva-nīly-a-samyag-vyadhādiṣu ।।

śliṣṭa-vartmany asṛk-srāve īly-a-samyag-vyadhādiṣu
sirādi-dāhas tair eva na dahet kṣāra-vāritān ।
antaḥ-śalyāsṛjo bhinna-koṣṭhān bhūri-vraṇāturān ।।

a dahet kṣāra-varjitān
su-dagdhaṃ ghṛta-madhv-aktaṃ snigdha-śītaiḥ pradehayet ।
tasya liṅgaṃ sthite rakte śabda-val lasikānvitam ।।

pakva-tāla-kapotābhaṃ su-rohaṃ nāti-vedanam ।
pramāda-dagdha-vat sarvaṃ dur-dagdhāty-artha-dagdhayoḥ ।।

catur-dhā tat tu tucchena saha tucchasya lakṣaṇam ।
tvag vi-varṇoṣyate aty-arthaṃ na ca sphoṭa-samudbhavaḥ ।।

atur-dhā tac ca tucchena atur-dhā tat tu tutthena atur-dhā tatra tucchena 
aha tutthasya lakṣaṇam
sa-sphoṭa-dāha-tīvroṣaṃ dur-dagdham ati-dāhataḥ ।
māṃsa-lambana-saṃkoca-dāha-dhūpana-vedanāḥ ।।

sirādi-nāśas tṛṇ-mūrchā-vraṇa-gāmbhīrya-mṛtyavaḥ ।
tucchasyāgni-pratapanaṃ kāryam uṣṇaṃ ca bheṣajam ।।

irādi-nāśa-tṛṇ-mūrchā- utthasyāgni-pratapanaṃ
styāne asre vedanāty-arthaṃ vilīne manda-tā rujaḥ ।
dur-dagdhe śītam uṣṇaṃ ca yuñjyād ādau tato himam ।।

samyag-dagdhe tavakṣīrī-plakṣa-candana-gairikaiḥ ।
limpet sājyāmṛtair ūrdhvaṃ pitta-vidradhi-vat kriyā ।।

amyag-dagdhe tukākṣīrī- itta-vidradhi-vat kriyām 
pitta-vidradhi-vat kriyāḥ
ati-dagdhe drutaṃ kuryāt sarvaṃ pitta-visarpa-vat ।
sneha-dagdhe bhṛśa-taraṃ rūkṣaṃ tatra tu yojayet ।।

śastra-kṣārāgnayo yasmān mṛtyoḥ paramam āyudham ।
a-pramatto bhiṣak tasmāt tān samyag avacārayet ।।

tat samyag avacārayet
samāpyate sthānam idaṃ hṛdayasya rahasya-vat ।
atrārthāḥ sūtritāḥ sūkṣmāḥ pratanyante hi sarvataḥ ।।

trārthāḥ sūcitāḥ sūkṣmāḥ

”ārīrasthāna
śuddhe śukrārtave sat-tvaḥ sva-karma-kleśa-coditaḥ ।
garbhaḥ saṃpadyate yukti-vaśād agnir ivāraṇau ।।

va-karma-phala-noditaḥ
bījātmakair mahā-bhūtaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ sat-tvānugaiś ca saḥ ।
mātuś cāhāra-rasa-jaiḥ kramāt kukṣau vivardhate ।।

tejo yathārka-raśmīnāṃ sphaṭikena tiras-kṛtam ।
nendhanaṃ dṛśyate gacchat sat-tvo garbhāśayaṃ tathā ।।

kāraṇānuvidhāyi-tvāt kāryāṇāṃ tat-sva-bhāva-tā ।
nānā-yony-ākṛtīḥ sat-tvo dhatte ato druta-loha-vat ।।

ata eva ca śukrasya bāhulyāj jāyate pumān ।
raktasya strī tayoḥ sāmye klībaḥ śukrārtave punaḥ ।।

vāyunā bahu-śo bhinne yathā-svaṃ bahv-apatya-tā ।
vi-yoni-vikṛtākārā jāyante vikṛtair malaiḥ ।।

māsi māsi rajaḥ strīṇāṃ rasa-jaṃ sravati try-aham ।
vatsarād dvā-daśād ūrdhvaṃ yāti pañcāśataḥ kṣayam ।।

pūrṇa-ṣo-ḍaśa-varṣā strī pūrṇa-viṃśena saṃgatā ।
śuddhe garbhāśaye mārge rakte śukre anile hṛdi ।।

vīrya-vantaṃ sutaṃ sūte tato nyūnābdayoḥ punaḥ ।
rogy alpāyur a-dhanyo vā garbho bhavati naiva vā ।।

vātādi-kuṇapa-granthi-pūya-kṣīṇa-malāhvayam ।
bījā-samarthaṃ reto-'sraṃ sva-liṅgair doṣa-jaṃ vadet ।।

rajā-samarthaṃ reto-'sraṃ
raktena kuṇapaṃ śleṣma-vātābhyāṃ granthi-saṃnibham ।
pūyābhaṃ rakta-pittābhyāṃ kṣīṇaṃ māruta-pittataḥ ।।

kṛcchrāṇy etāny a-sādhyaṃ tu tri-doṣaṃ mūtra-viṭ-prabham ।
kuryād vātādibhir duṣṭe svauṣadhaṃ kuṇape punaḥ ।।

dhātakī-puṣpa-khadira-dāḍimārjuna-sādhitam ।
pāyayet sarpir atha-vā vipakvam asanādibhiḥ ।।

palāśa-bhasmāśmabhidā granthy-ābhe pūya-retasi ।
parūṣaka-vaṭādibhyāṃ kṣīṇe śukra-karī kriyā ।।

snigdhaṃ vāntaṃ viriktaṃ ca nirūḍham anuvāsitam ।
yojayec chukra-doṣārtaṃ samyag uttara-vastibhiḥ ।।

saṃśuddho viṭ-prabhe sarpir hiṅgu-sevyādi-sādhitam ।
pibed granthy-ārtave pāṭhā-vyoṣa-vṛkṣaka-jaṃ jalam ।।

iṅgu-sevyāgni-sādhitam
peyaṃ kuṇapa-pūyāsre candanaṃ vakṣyate tu yat ।
guhya-roge ca tat sarvaṃ kāryaṃ sottara-vastikam ।।

śukraṃ śuklaṃ guru snigdhaṃ madhuraṃ bahalaṃ bahu ।
ghṛta-mākṣika-tailābhaṃ sad-garbhāyārtavaṃ punaḥ ।।

śuddhaṃ śukraṃ guru snigdhaṃ
lākṣā-rasa-śaśāsrābhaṃ dhautaṃ yac ca virajyate ।
śuddha-śukrārtavaṃ svasthaṃ saṃraktaṃ mithunaṃ mithaḥ ।।

snehaiḥ puṃ-savanaiḥ snigdhaṃ śuddhaṃ śīlita-vastikam ।
naraṃ viśeṣāt kṣīrājyair madhurauṣadha-saṃskṛtaiḥ ।।

adhurauṣadha-sādhitaiḥ
nārīṃ tailena māṣaiś ca pittalaiḥ samupācaret ।
kṣāma-prasanna-vadanāṃ sphurac-chroṇi-payo-dharām ।।

ṣāmāṃ prasanna-vadanāṃ
srastākṣi-kukṣiṃ puṃs-kāmāṃ vidyād ṛtu-matīṃ striyam ।
padmaṃ saṃkocam āyāti dine atīte yathā tathā ।।

ṛtāv atīte yoniḥ sā śukraṃ nātaḥ pratīcchati ।
māsenopacitaṃ raktaṃ dhamanībhyām ṛtau punaḥ ।।

śukraṃ nāntaḥ pratīcchati
īṣat-kṛṣṇaṃ vi-gandhaṃ ca vāyur yoni-mukhān nudet ।
tataḥ puṣpekṣaṇād eva kalyāṇa-dhyāyinī try-aham ।।

mṛjālaṅkāra-rahitā darbha-saṃstara-śāyinī ।
kṣaireyaṃ yāvakaṃ stokaṃ koṣṭha-śodhana-karṣaṇam ।।

oṣṭha-śodhana-karśanam
parṇe śarāve haste vā bhuñjīta brahma-cāriṇī ।
caturthe ahni tataḥ snātā śukla-mālyāmbarā śuciḥ ।।

icchantī bhartṛ-sadṛśaṃ putraṃ paśyet puraḥ patim ।
ṛtus tu dvā-daśa niśāḥ pūrvās tisro atra ninditāḥ ।।

ūrvās tisraś ca ninditāḥ
ekā-daśī ca yugmāsu syāt putro anyāsu kanyakā ।
upādhyāyo atha putrīyaṃ kurvīta vidhi-vad vidhim ।।

yāt putro anya-tra kanyakā
namas-kāra-parāyās tu śūdrāyā mantra-varjitam ।
a-vandhya evaṃ saṃyogaḥ syād apatyaṃ ca kāmataḥ ।।

santo hy āhur apatyārthaṃ dam-patyoḥ saṃgatiṃ rahaḥ ।
dur-apatyaṃ kulāṅgāro gotre jātaṃ mahaty api ।।

am-patyoḥ saṃgataṃ rahaḥ ur-apatyaṃ kulāṅgāraṃ
icchetāṃ yādṛśaṃ putraṃ tad-rūpa-caritāṃś ca tau ।
cintayetāṃ jana-padāṃs tad-ācāra-paricchadau ।।

karmānte ca pumān sarpiḥ-kṣīra-śāly-odanāśitaḥ ।
prāg dakṣiṇena pādena śayyāṃ mauhūrtikājñayā ।।

ārohet strī tu vāmena tasya dakṣiṇa-pārśvataḥ ।
taila-māṣottarāhārā tatra mantr aṃ prayojayet ।।

ārohet strī ca vāmena āhir asy āyur asi sarvataḥ pratiṣṭhāsi ।।

hir asi sarvataḥ pratiṣṭhāsi dhātā tvāṃ dadhātu vidhātā tvāṃ dadhātu ।।
brahma-varcasā bhaveti ।।
rahma-varcasā bhaved iti
brahmā bṛhaspatir viṣṇuḥ somaḥ sūryas tathāśvinau ।
bhago atha mitrā-varuṇau vīraṃ dadatu me sutam ।।

sāntvayitvā tato anya-nyaṃ saṃviśetāṃ mudānvitau ।
uttānā tan-manā yoṣit tiṣṭhed aṅgaiḥ su-saṃsthitaiḥ ।।

āntayitvā tato anyo-'nyaṃ aṃvasetāṃ mudānvitau
tathā hi bījaṃ gṛhṇāti doṣaiḥ sva-sthānam āsthitaiḥ ।
liṅgaṃ tu sadyo-garbhāyā yonyā bījasya saṃgrahaḥ ।।

oṣaiḥ sva-sthānam āśritaiḥ onyāṃ bījasya saṃgrahaḥ
tṛptir guru-tvaṃ sphuraṇaṃ śukrāsrān-anu bandhanam ।
hṛdaya-spandanaṃ tandrā tṛḍ glānī roma-harṣaṇam ।।

a-vyaktaḥ prathame māsi saptāhāt kalalī-bhavet ।
garbhaḥ puṃ-savanāny atra pūrvaṃ vyakteḥ prayojayet ।।

balī puruṣa-kāro hi daivam apy ativartate ।
puṣye puruṣakaṃ haimaṃ rājataṃ vātha-vāyasam ।।

kṛtvāgni-varṇaṃ nirvāpya kṣīre tasyāñjaliṃ pibet ।
gauradaṇḍam apāmārgaṃ jīvakarṣabha-sairyakān ।।

pibet puṣye jale piṣṭān eka-dvi-tri-samasta-śaḥ ।
kṣīreṇa śveta-bṛhatī-mūlaṃ nāsā-puṭe svayam ।।

putrārthaṃ dakṣiṇe siñced vāme duhitṛ-vāñchayā ।
payasā lakṣmaṇā-mūlaṃ putrotpāda-sthiti-pradam ।।

nāsayāsyena vā pītaṃ vaṭa-śuṅgāṣṭakaṃ tathā ।
oṣadhīr jīvanīyāś ca bāhyāntar upayojayet ।।

aṭa-śṛṅgāṣṭakaṃ tathā
upacāraḥ priya-hitair bhartrā bhṛtyaiś ca garbha-dhṛk ।
nava-nīta-ghṛta-kṣīraiḥ sadā cainām upācaret ।।

ati-vyavāyam āyāsaṃ bhāraṃ prāvaraṇaṃ guru ।
a-kāla-jāgara-svapnaṃ kaṭhinotkaṭakāsanam ।।

ti-vyavāyaṃ vyāyāmaṃ -kāla-jāgara-svapna- -kaṭhinotkaṭakāsanam 
aṭhinotkaṭukāsanam -kaṭhinotkuṭakāsanam
śoka-krodha-bhayodvega-vega-śraddhā-vidhāraṇam ।
upavāsādhva-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-guru-viṣṭambhi-bhojanam ।।

pavāsādi-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-
raktaṃ nivasanaṃ śvabhra-kūpekṣāṃ madyam āmiṣam ।
uttāna-śayanaṃ yac ca striyo necchanti tat tyajet ।।

aktaṃ vi-vasanaṃ śvabhra-
tathā rakta-srutiṃ śuddhiṃ vastim ā-māsato aṣṭamāt ।
ebhir garbhaḥ sraved āmaḥ kukṣau śuṣyen mriyeta vā ।।

vaṃ garbhaḥ sraved āmaḥ
vātalaiś ca bhaved garbhaḥ kubjāndha-jaḍa-vāmanaḥ ।
pittalaiḥ khalatiḥ piṅgaḥ śvitrī pāṇḍuḥ kaphātmabhiḥ ।।

vyādhīṃś cāsyā mṛdu-sukhair a-tīkṣṇair auṣadhair jayet ।
dvitīye māsi kalalād ghanaḥ peśy atha-vārbudam ।।

puṃ-strī-klībāḥ kramāt tebhyas tatra vyaktasya lakṣaṇam ।
kṣāma-tā garimā kukṣer mūrchā chardir a-rocakaḥ ।।

ṣāma-tā garimā kukṣau
jṛmbhā prasekaḥ sadanaṃ roma-rājyāḥ prakāśanam ।
amleṣṭa-tā stanau pīnau sa-stanyau kṛṣṇa-cūcukau ।।

pāda-śopho vidāho anye śraddhāś ca vividhātmikāḥ ।
mātṛ-jaṃ hy asya hṛdayaṃ mātuś ca hṛdayena tat ।।

āda-śopho vidāho anne
saṃbaddhaṃ tena garbhiṇyā neṣṭaṃ śraddhā-vimānanam ।
deyam apy a-hitaṃ tasyai hitopahitam alpakam ।।

eṣṭaṃ śraddhā-vidhāraṇam eṣṭaṃ śraddhāvamānanam
śraddhā-vighātād garbhasya vikṛtiś cyutir eva vā ।
vyaktī-bhavati māse asya tṛtīye gātra-pañcakam ।।

śraddhābhighātād garbhasya
mūrdhā dve sakthinī bāhū sarva-sūkṣmāṅga-janma ca ।
samam eva hi mūrdhādyair jñānaṃ ca sukha-duḥkhayoḥ ।।

arva-sūkṣmāṅga-janma tu ijñānaṃ sukha-duḥkhayoḥ
garbhasya nābhau mātuś ca hṛdi nāḍī nibadhyate ।
yayā sa puṣṭim āpnoti kedāra iva kulyayā ।।

ayā puṣṭim avāpnoti
caturthe vyakta-tāṅgānāṃ cetanāyāś ca pañcame ।
ṣaṣṭhe snāyu-sirā-roma-bala-varṇa-nakha-tvacām ।।
sarvaiḥ sarvāṅga-saṃpūrṇo bhāvaiḥ puṣyati saptame ।।garbheṇotpīḍitā doṣās tasmin hṛdayam āśritāḥ ।।kaṇḍūṃ vidāhaṃ kurvanti garbhiṇyāḥ kikkisāni ca ।।
nava-nītaṃ hitaṃ tatra kolāmbu-madhurauṣadhaiḥ ।
siddham alpa-paṭu-snehaṃ laghu svādu ca bhojanam ।।

candanośīra-kalkena limped ūru-stanodaram ।
śreṣṭhayā vaiṇa-hariṇa-śaśa-śoṇita-yuktayā ।।

aśvaghna-pattra-siddhena tailenābhyajya mardayet ।
paṭola-nimba-mañjiṣṭhā-surasaiḥ secayet punaḥ ।।

dārvī-madhuka-toyena mṛjāṃ ca pariśīlayet ।
ojo aṣṭame saṃcarati mātā-putrau muhuḥ kramāt ।।

tena tau mlāna-muditau tatra jāto na jīvati ।
śiśur ojo-'n-avasthānān nārī saṃśayitā bhavet ।।

yātām atra na jīvati yātāṃ jāto na jīvati
kṣīra-peyā ca peyātra sa-ghṛtānvāsanaṃ ghṛtam ।
madhuraiḥ sādhitaṃ śuddhyai purāṇa-śakṛtas tathā ।।

a-ghṛtānvāsanaṃ hitam
śuṣka-mūlaka-kolāmla-kaṣāyeṇa praśasyate ।
śatāhvā-kalkito vastiḥ sa-taila-ghṛta-saindhavaḥ ।।

tasmiṃs tv ekāha-yāte api kālaḥ sūter ataḥ param ।
varṣād vikāra-kārī syāt kukṣau vātena dhāritaḥ ।।

asminn ekāha-yāte api
śastaś ca navame māsi snigdho māṃsa-rasaudanaḥ ।
bahu-snehā yavāgūr vā pūrvoktaṃ cānuvāsanam ।।

nigdha-māṃsa-rasaudanaḥ
tata eva picuṃ cāsyā yonau nityaṃ nidhāpayet ।
vāta-ghna-pattra-bhaṅgāmbhaḥ śītaṃ snāne anv-ahaṃ hitam ।।

niḥ-snehāṅgī na navamān māsāt prabhṛti vāsayet ।
prāg dakṣiṇa-stana-stanyā pūrvaṃ tat-pārśva-ceṣṭinī ।।

puṃ-nāma-daurhṛda-praśna-ratā puṃ-svapna-darśinī ।
unnate dakṣiṇe kukṣau garbhe ca parimaṇḍale ।।

putraṃ sūte anya-thā kanyāṃ yā cecchati nṛ-saṃgatim ।
nṛtya-vāditra-gāndharva-gandha-mālya-priyā ca yā ।।

klībaṃ tat-saṃkare tatra madhyaṃ kukṣeḥ samunnatam ।
yamau pārśva-dvayonnāmāt kukṣau droṇyām iva sthite ।।

prāk caiva navamān māsāt sā sūti-gṛham āśrayet ।
deśe praśaste saṃbhāraiḥ saṃpannaṃ sādhake ahani ।।

ūtikā-gṛham āśrayet
tatrodīkṣeta sā sūtiṃ sūtikā-parivāritā ।
adya-śvaḥ-prasave glāniḥ kukṣy-akṣi-ślatha-tā klamaḥ ।।

āsanna-prasave glāniḥ
adho-guru-tvam a-ruciḥ praseko bahu-mūtra-tā ।
vedanorūdara-kaṭī-pṛṣṭha-hṛd-vasti-vaṅkṣaṇe ।।

yoni-bheda-rujā-toda-sphuraṇa-sravaṇāni ca ।
āvīnām anu janmātas tato garbhodaka-srutiḥ ।।

athopasthita-garbhāṃ tāṃ kṛta-kautuka-magalām ।
hasta-stha-puṃ-nāma-phalāṃ sv-abhyaktoṣṇāmbu-secitām ।।

v-aktām uṣṇāmbu-secitām
pāyayet sa-ghṛtāṃ peyāṃ tanau bhū-śayane sthitām ।
ābhugna-sakthim uttānām abhyaktāṅgīṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।।

adho nābher vimṛdnīyāt kārayej jṛmbha-caṅkramam ।
garbhaḥ prayāty avāg evaṃ tal-liṅgaṃ hṛd-vimokṣataḥ ।।

āviśya jaṭharaṃ garbho vaster upari tiṣṭhati ।
āvyo abhitvarayanty enāṃ khaṭvām āropayet tataḥ ।।

āvyo hi tvarayanty enāṃ
atha saṃpīḍite garbhe yonim asyāḥ prasārayet ।
mṛdu pūrvaṃ pravāheta bāḍham ā-prasavāc ca sā ।।

onim asyāḥ prasādhayet
harṣayet tāṃ muhuḥ putra-janma-śabda-jalānilaiḥ ।
pratyāyānti tathā prāṇāḥ sūti-kleśāvasāditāḥ ।।

dhūpayed garbha-saṅge tu yoniṃ kṛṣṇāhi-kañcukaiḥ ।
hiraṇyapuṣpī-mūlaṃ ca pāṇi-pādena dhārayet ।।

suvarcalāṃ viśalyāṃ vā jarāyv-a-patane api ca ।
kāryam etat tathotkṣipya bāhvor enāṃ vikampayet ।।

āryam etat tathotkṛṣya āhvor etāṃ vikampayet
kaṭīm ākoṭayet pārṣṇyā sphijau gāḍhaṃ nipīḍayet ।
tālu-kaṇṭhaṃ spṛśed veṇyā mūrdhni dadyāt snuhī-payaḥ ।।

bhūrja-lāṅgalikī-tumbī-sarpa-tvak-kuṣṭha-sarṣapaiḥ ।
pṛthag dvābhyāṃ samastair vā yoni-lepana-dhūpanam ।।

oni-dhūpaṃ ca lepanam
kuṣṭha-tālīśa-kalkaṃ vā surā-maṇḍena pāyayet ।
yūṣeṇa vā kulatthānāṃ bālbajenāsavena vā ।।

ilva-jenāsavena vā
śatāhvā-sarṣapājājī-śigru-tīkṣṇaka-citrakaiḥ ।
sa-hiṅgu-kuṣṭha-madanair mūtre kṣīre ca sārṣapam ।।

tailaṃ siddhaṃ hitaṃ pāyau yonyāṃ vāpy anuvāsanam ।
śatapuṣpā-vacā-kuṣṭha-kaṇā-sarṣapa-kalkitaḥ ।।

onyāṃ vā hy anuvāsanam
nirūhaḥ pātayaty āśu sa-sneha-lavaṇo aparām ।
tat-saṅge hy anilo hetuḥ sā niryāty āśu taj-jayāt ।।

kuśalā pāṇināktena haret kḷpta-nakhena vā ।
mukta-garbhāparāṃ yoniṃ tailenāṅgaṃ ca mardayet ।।

makkallākhye śiro-vasti-koṣṭha-śūle tu pāyayet ।
su-cūrṇitaṃ yava-kṣāraṃ ghṛtenoṣṇa-jalena vā ।।

dhānyāmbu vā guḍa-vyoṣa-tri-jātaka-rajo-'nvitam ।
atha bālopacāreṇa bālaṃ yoṣid upācared ।।

sūtikā kṣud-vatī tailād ghṛtād vā mahatīṃ pibet ।
pañca-kolakinīṃ mātrām anu coṣṇaṃ guḍodakam ।।

vāta-ghnauṣadha-toyaṃ vā tathā vāyur na kupyati ।
viśudhyati ca duṣṭāsraṃ dvi-tri-rātram ayaṃ kramaḥ ।।

athā vāyur na kupyati
snehā-yogyā tu niḥ-sneham amum eva vidhiṃ bhajet ।
pīta-vatyāś ca jaṭharaṃ yamakāktaṃ viveṣṭayet ।।

jīrṇe snātā pibet peyāṃ pūrvoktauṣadha-sādhitām ।
try-ahād ūrdhvaṃ vidāry-ādi-varga-kvāthena sādhitā ।।

hitā yavāgūḥ snehāḍhyā sātmyataḥ payasātha-vā ।
sapta-rātrāt paraṃ cāsyai krama-śo bṛṃhaṇaṃ hitam ।।

apta-rātrāt paraṃ cāsyāḥ apta-rātrāt paraṃ vāsyāḥ
dvā-daśāhe an-atikrānte piśitaṃ nopayojayet ।
yatnenopacaret sūtāṃ duḥ-sādhyo hi tad-āmayaḥ ।।

iśitaṃ naiva yojayet
garbha-vṛddhi-prasava-ruk-kledāsra-sruti-pīḍanaiḥ ।
evaṃ ca māsād adhy-ardhān muktāhārādi-yantraṇā ।।
gata-sūtābhidhānā syāt punar ārtava-darśanāt ।।
”ārīrasthāna
garbhiṇyāḥ parihāryāṇāṃ sevayā rogato atha-vā ।
puṣpe dṛṣṭe atha-vā śūle bāhyāntaḥ snigdha-śītalam ।।

evayā rogato api vā
sevyāmbho-ja-hima-kṣīri-valka-kalkājya-lepitān ।
dhārayed yoni-vastibhyām ārdrārdrān picu-naktakān ।।

hārayed vasti-yonibhyām
śata-dhauta-ghṛtāktāṃ strīṃ tad-ambhasy avagāhayet ।
sa-sitā-kṣaudra-kumuda-kamalotpala-kesaram ।।

lihyāt kṣīra-ghṛtaṃ khādec chṛṅgāṭaka-kaserukam ।
pibet kāntāb-ja-śālūka-bālodumbara-vat payaḥ ।।

śṛtena śāli-kākolī-dvi-balā-madhukekṣubhiḥ ।
payasā rakta-śāly-annam adyāt sa-madhu-śarkaram ।।

rasair vā jāṅgalaiḥ śuddhi-varjaṃ cāsroktam ācaret ।
a-saṃpūrṇa-tri-māsāyāḥ pratyākhyāya prasādhayet ।।

-varjaṃ vāsroktam ācaret
āmānvaye ca tatreṣṭaṃ śītaṃ rūkṣopasaṃhitam ।
upavāso ghanośīra-guḍūcy-aralu-dhānyakāḥ ।।

durālabhā-parpaṭaka-candanātiviṣā-balāḥ ।
kvathitāḥ salile pānaṃ tṛṇa-dhānyāni bhojanam ।।

ṛṇa-dhānyādi bhojanam
mudgādi-yūṣair āme tu jite snigdhādi pūrva-vat ।
garbhe nipatite tīkṣṇaṃ madyaṃ sāmarthyataḥ pibet ।।

garbha-koṣṭha-viśuddhy-artham arti-vismaraṇāya ca ।
laghunā pañca-mūlena rūkṣāṃ peyāṃ tataḥ pibet ।।

peyām a-madya-pā kalke sādhitāṃ pāñcakaulike ।
bilvādi-pañcaka-kvāthe tiloddālaka-taṇḍulaiḥ ।।

māsa-tulya-dināny evaṃ peyādiḥ patite kramaḥ ।
laghur a-sneha-lavaṇo dīpanīya-yuto hitaḥ ।।

īpanīya-yuto hi saḥ
doṣa-dhātu-parikleda-śoṣārthaṃ vidhir ity ayam ।
snehānna-vastayaś cordhvaṃ balya-dīpana-jīvanāḥ ।।

saṃjāta-sāre mahati garbhe yoni-parisravāt ।
vṛddhim a-prāpnuvan garbhaḥ koṣṭhe tiṣṭhati sa-sphuraḥ ।।

upaviṣṭakam āhus taṃ vardhate tena nodaram ।
śokopavāsa-rūkṣādyair atha-vā yony-ati-sravāt ।।

vāte kruddhe kṛśaḥ śuṣyed garbho nāgodaraṃ tu tam ।
udaraṃ vṛddham apy atra hīyate sphuraṇaṃ cirāt ।।

arbho nāgodaraṃ tu tat
tayor bṛṃhaṇa-vāta-ghna-madhura-dravya-saṃskṛtaiḥ ।
ghṛta-kṣīra-rasais tṛptir āma-garbhāṃś ca khādayet ।।

tair eva ca su-bhikṣāyāḥ kṣobhaṇaṃ yāna-vāhanaiḥ ।
līnākhye nisphure śyena-go-matsyotkrośa-barhi-jāḥ ।।

air eva ca su-tṛptāyāḥ
rasā bahu-ghṛtā deyā māṣa-mūlaka-jā api ।
bāla-bilvaṃ tilān māṣān saktūṃś ca payasā pibet ।।

sa-medya-māṃsaṃ madhu vā kaṭy-abhyaṅgaṃ ca śīlayet ।
harṣayet satataṃ cainām evaṃ garbhaḥ pravardhate ।।

puṣṭo anya-thā varṣa-gaṇaiḥ kṛcchrāj jāyeta naiva vā ।
udāvartaṃ tu garbhiṇyāḥ snehair āśu-tarāṃ jayet ।।

yogyaiś ca vastibhir hanyāt sa-garbhāṃ sa hi garbhiṇīm ।
garbhe ati-doṣopacayād a-pathyair daivato api vā ।।

mṛte antar udaraṃ śītaṃ stabdhaṃ dhmātaṃ bhṛśa-vyatham ।
garbhā-spando bhrama-tṛṣṇā kṛcchrād ucchvasanaṃ klamaḥ ।।

ṛte antar jaṭharaṃ śītaṃ tabdhādhmātaṃ bhṛśa-vyatham
a-ratiḥ srasta-netra-tvam āvīnām a-samudbhavaḥ ।
tasyāḥ koṣṇāmbu-siktāyāḥ piṣṭvā yoniṃ pralepayet ।।

guḍaṃ kiṇvaṃ sa-lavaṇaṃ tathāntaḥ pūrayen muhuḥ ।
ghṛtena kalkī-kṛtayā śālmaly-atasi-picchayā ।।

mantrair yogair jarāyūktair mūḍha-garbho na cet patet ।
athāpṛcchyeśvaraṃ vaidyo yatnenāśu tam āharet ।।

tha pṛṣṭveśvaraṃ vaidyo thāpṛṣṭveśvaraṃ vaidyo
hastam abhyajya yoniṃ ca sājya-śālmali-picchayā ।
hastena śakyaṃ tenaiva gātraṃ ca viṣamaṃ sthitam ।।

ātraṃ ca viṣama-sthitam
āñchanotpīḍa-saṃpīḍa-vikṣepotkṣepaṇādibhiḥ ।
ānulomya samākarṣed yoniṃ praty ārjavāgatam ।।

ānulomye samākarṣed
hasta-pāda-śirobhir yo yoniṃ bhugnaḥ prapadyate ।
pādena yonim ekena bhugno anyena gudaṃ ca yaḥ ।।

viṣkambhau nāma tau mūḍhau śastra-dāraṇam arhataḥ ।
maṇḍalāṅguli-śastrābhyāṃ tatra karma praśasyate ।।

vṛddhi-pattraṃ hi tīkṣṇāgraṃ na yonāv avacārayet ।
pūrvaṃ śiraḥ-kapālāni dārayitvā viśodhayet ।।

kakṣoras-tālu-cibuka-pradeśe anya-tame tataḥ ।
samālambya dṛḍhaṃ karṣet kuśalo garbha-śaṅkunā ।।

akṣoras-tālu-cibuke radeśe anya-tame tataḥ
a-bhinna-śirasaṃ tv akṣi-kūṭayor gaṇḍayor api ।
bāhuṃ chittvāṃsa-saktasya vātādhmātodarasya tu ।।

vidārya koṣṭham antrāṇi bahir vā saṃnirasya ca ।
kaṭī-saktasya tad-vac ca tat-kapālāni dārayet ।।

yad yad vāyu-vaśād aṅgaṃ sajjed garbhasya khaṇḍa-śaḥ ।
tat tac chittvāharet samyag rakṣen nārīṃ ca yatnataḥ ।।

at tac chittvāharan samyag
garbhasya hi gatiṃ citrāṃ karoti vi-guṇo anilaḥ ।
tatrān-alpa-matis tasmād avasthāpekṣam ācaret ।।

chindyād garbhaṃ na jīvantaṃ mātaraṃ sa hi mārayet ।
sahātmanā na copekṣyaḥ kṣaṇam apy asta-jīvitaḥ ।।

yoni-saṃvaraṇa-bhraṃśa-makkalla-śvāsa-pīḍitām ।
pūty-udgārāṃ himāṅgīṃ ca mūḍha-garbhāṃ parityajet ।।

athā-patantīm aparāṃ pātayet pūrva-vad bhiṣak ।
evaṃ nirhṛta-śalyāṃ tu siñced uṣṇena vāriṇā ।।

dadyād abhyakta-dehāyai yonau sneha-picuṃ tataḥ ।
yonir mṛdur bhavet tena śūlaṃ cāsyāḥ praśāmyati ।।

dīpyakātiviṣā-rāsnā-hiṅgv-elā-pañca-kolakāt ।
cūrṇaṃ snehena kalkaṃ vā kvāthaṃ vā pāyayet tataḥ ।।

vāthaṃ tāṃ pāyayet tataḥ
kaṭukātiviṣā-pāṭhā-śāka-tvag-ghiṅgu-tejinīḥ ।
tad-vac ca doṣa-syandārthaṃ vedanopaśamāya ca ।।

-śāka-tvag-ghiṅgu-tejanīḥ
tri-rātram evaṃ saptāhaṃ sneham eva tataḥ pibet ।
sāyaṃ pibed ariṣṭaṃ ca tathā su-kṛtam āsavam ।।

śirīṣa-kakubha-kvātha-picūn yonau vinikṣipet ।
upadravāś ca ye anye syus tān yathā-svam upācaret ।।

payo vāta-haraiḥ siddhaṃ daśāhaṃ bhojane hitam ।
raso daśāhaṃ ca paraṃ laghu-pathyālpa-bhojanā ।।

svedābhyaṅga-parā snehān balā-tailādikān bhajet ।
ūrdhvaṃ caturbhyo māsebhyaḥ sā krameṇa sukhāni ca ।।

balā-mūla-kaṣāyasya bhāgāḥ ṣaṭ payasas tathā ।
yava-kola-kulatthānāṃ daśa-mūlasya caikataḥ ।।

niḥkvātha-bhāgo bhāgaś ca tailasya tu catur-daśaḥ ।
dvi-medā-dāru-mañjiṣṭhā-kākolī-dvaya-candanaiḥ ।।

ailasya ca catur-daśaḥ
śārivā-kuṣṭha-tagara-jīvakarṣabha-saindhavaiḥ ।
kālānusāryā-śaileya-vacāguru-punarnavaiḥ ।।

ālānusārī-śaileya- ālānusārya-śaileya-
aśvagandhā-varī-kṣīraśuklā-yaṣṭī-varā-rasaiḥ ।
śatāhvā-śūrpaparṇy-elā-tvak-pattraiḥ ślakṣṇa-kalkitaiḥ ।।

pakvaṃ mṛdv-agninā tailaṃ sarva-vāta-vikāra-jit ।
sūtikā-bāla-marmāsthi-hata-kṣīṇeṣu pūjitam ।।

-kṣata-kṣīṇeṣu pūjitam
jvara-gulma-grahonmāda-mūtrāghātāntra-vṛddhi-jit ।
dhanvantarer abhimataṃ yoni-roga-kṣayāpaham ।।

vasti-dvāre vipannāyāḥ kukṣiḥ praspandate yadi ।
janma-kāle tataḥ śīghraṃ pāṭayitvoddharec chiśum ।।

madhukaṃ śāka-bījaṃ ca payasyā suradāru ca ।
aśmantakaḥ kṛṣṇa-tilās tāmravallī śatāvarī ।।

ayasyāmaradāru ca
vṛkṣādanī payasyā ca latā sotpala-śārivā ।
anantā śārivā rāsnā padmā ca madhuyaṣṭikā ।।

atā cotpala-śārivā admātha madhuyaṣṭikā admāhva-madhuyaṣṭikā 
admakaṃ madhuyaṣṭikā
bṛhatī-dvaya-kāśmarya-kṣīri-śuṅga-tvacā ghṛtam ।
pṛśniparṇī balā śigruḥ śvadaṃṣṭrā madhuparṇikā ।।

ṛhatī-dvaya-kāśmaryaḥ -kṣīri-śṛṅga-tvacā ghṛtam 
kṣīri-śuṅga-tvacā ghṛtam
śṛṅgāṭakaṃ bisaṃ drākṣā kaseru madhukaṃ sitā ।
saptaitān payasā yogān ardha-śloka-samāpanān ।।

kramāt saptasu māseṣu garbhe sravati yojayet ।
kapittha-bilva-bṛhatī-paṭolekṣu-nidigdhikāt ।।

-paṭolekṣu-nidigdhi-jaiḥ
mūlaiḥ śṛtaṃ prayuñjīta kṣīraṃ māse tathāṣṭame ।
navame śārivānantā-payasyā-madhuyaṣṭibhiḥ ।।

yojayed daśame māsi siddhaṃ kṣīraṃ payasyayā ।
atha-vā yaṣṭimadhuka-nāgarāmaradārubhiḥ ।।

avasthitaṃ lohitam aṅganāyā vātena garbhaṃ bruvate an-abhijñāḥ ।
garbhākṛti-tvāt kaṭukoṣṇa-tīkṣṇaiḥ srute punaḥ kevala eva rakte ।।

garbhaṃ jaḍā bhūta-hṛtaṃ vadanti mūrter na dṛṣṭaṃ haraṇaṃ yatas taiḥ ।
ojo-'śana-tvād atha-vā-vyavasthair bhūtair upekṣyeta na garbha-mātā ।।

”ārīrasthāna
śiro antar-ādhir dvau bāhū sakthinīti samāsataḥ ।
ṣaḍ-aṅgam aṅgaṃ pratyaṅgaṃ tasyākṣi-hṛdayādikam ।।

akthinī ca samāsataḥ
śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaḥ kramād guṇāḥ ।
khānilāgny-ab-bhuvām eka-guṇa-vṛddhy-anvayaḥ pare ।।

hānilāgny-ambu-bhūṣv eka- -guṇa-vṛddhyānvayaḥ pare
tatra khāt khāni dehe asmin śrotraṃ śabdo vivikta-tā ।
vātāt sparśa-tvag-ucchvāsā vahner dṛg-rūpa-paktayaḥ ।।

āpyā jihvā-rasa-kledā ghrāṇa-gandhāsthi pārthivam ।
mṛatra mātṛ-jaṃ rakta-māṃsa-majja-gudādikam ।।

paitṛkaṃ tu sthiraṃ śukra-dhamany-asthi-kacādikam ।
caitanaṃ cittam akṣāṇi nānā-yoniṣu janma ca ।।

ātma-jaṃ cittaṃ akṣāṇi
sātmya-jaṃ tv āyur ārogyam an-ālasyaṃ prabhā balam ।
rasa-jaṃ vapuṣo janma vṛttir vṛddhir a-lola-tā ।।

ātmya-jaṃ cāyur ārogyam
sāttvikaṃ śaucam āstikyaṃ śukla-dharma-rucir matiḥ ।
rājasaṃ bahu-bhāṣi-tvaṃ māna-krud-dambha-matsaram ।।

āna-krud-dambha-matsarāḥ
tāmasaṃ bhayam a-jñānaṃ nidrālasyaṃ viṣādi-tā ।
iti bhūta-mayo dehas tatra sapta tvaco asṛjaḥ ।।

pacyamānāt prajāyante kṣīrāt saṃtānikā iva ।
dhātv-āśayāntara-kledo vipakvaḥ svaṃ svam ūṣmaṇā ।।

śleṣma-snāyv-aparācchannaḥ kalākhyaḥ kāṣṭha-sāra-vat ।
tāḥ sapta sapta cādhārā raktasyādyaḥ kramāt pare ।।

c śleṣma-snāyv-aparā-channaḥ aktasyādhaḥ kramāt pare
kaphāma-pitta-pakvānāṃ vāyor mūtrasya ca smṛtāḥ ।
garbhāśayo aṣṭamaḥ strīṇāṃ pitta-pakvāśayāntare ।।

koṣṭhāṅgāni sthitāny eṣu hṛdayaṃ kloma phupphusam ।
yakṛt-plīhoṇḍukaṃ vṛkkau nābhi-ḍimbāntra-vastayaḥ ।।

ṛdayaṃ kloma phupphusaḥ ṛdayaṃ kloma-phupphuse
daśa jīvita-dhāmāni śiro-rasana-bandhanam ।
kaṇṭho asraṃ hṛdayaṃ nābhir vastiḥ śukraujasī gudam ।।

astiḥ śukraujasī gudaḥ
jālāni kaṇḍarāś cāṅge pṛthak ṣo-ḍaśa nirdiśet ।
ṣaṭ kūrcāḥ sapta sīvanyo meḍhra-jihvā-śiro-gatāḥ ।।

ṣaṭ kūrcāḥ sapta sevanyo ṣaṭ kūrcāḥ sapta sevinyo
śastreṇa tāḥ pariharec catasro māṃsa-rajjavaḥ ।
catur-daśāsthi-saṃghātāḥ sīmantā dvi-guṇā nava ।।

śastreṇaitāḥ pariharec
asthnāṃ śatāni ṣaṣṭiś ca trīṇi danta-nakhaiḥ saha ।
dhanvantaris tu trīṇy āha saṃdhīnāṃ ca śata-dvayam ।।

sthnāṃ śatāni ṣaṣṭhīni
daśottaraṃ sahasre dve nijagādātri-nandanaḥ ।
snāvnāṃ nava-śatī pañca puṃsāṃ peśī-śatāni tu ।।

nāyor nava-śatī pañca uṃsāṃ peśī-śatāni ca
adhikā viṃśatiḥ strīṇāṃ yoni-stana-samāśritāḥ ।
daśa mūla-sirā hṛt-sthās tāḥ sarvaṃ sarvato vapuḥ ।।

oni-stana-samāśrayāḥ
rasātmakaṃ vahanty ojas tan-nibaddhaṃ hi ceṣṭitam ।
sthūla-mūlāḥ su-sūkṣmāgrāḥ pattra-rekhā-pratāna-vat ।।

bhidyante tās tataḥ sapta-śatāny āsāṃ bhavanti tu ।
tatraikaikaṃ ca śākhāyāṃ śataṃ tasmin na vedhayet ।।

atraikaika-tra śākhāyāṃ
sirāṃ jālan-dharāṃ nāma tisraś cābhyantarāśritāḥ ।
ṣo-ḍaśa-dvi-guṇāḥ śroṇyāṃ tāsāṃ dve dve tu vaṅkṣaṇe ।।

dve dve kaṭīka-taruṇe śastreṇāṣṭau spṛśen na tāḥ ।
pārśvayoḥ ṣo-ḍaśaikaikām ūrdhva-gāṃ varjayet tayoḥ ।।

ūrdhva-gāṃ varjayet sirām
dvā-daśa-dvi-guṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe pṛṣṭha-vaṃśasya pārśvayoḥ ।
dve dve tatrordhva-gāminyau na śastreṇa parāmṛśet ।।

ṛṣṭha-vaṃśasya pārśva-ge
pṛṣṭha-vaj jaṭhare tāsāṃ mehanasyopari sthite ।
roma-rājīm ubhayato dve dve śastreṇa na spṛśet ।।

catvāriṃśad urasy āsāṃ catur-daśa na vedhayet ।
stana-rohita-tan-mūla-hṛdaye tu pṛthag dvayam ।।

apastambhākhyayor ekāṃ tathāpālāpayor api ।
grīvāyāṃ pṛṣṭha-vat tāsāṃ nīle manye kṛkāṭike ।।

vidhure mātṛkāś cāṣṭau ṣo-ḍaśeti parityajet ।
hanvoḥ ṣo-ḍaśa tāsāṃ dve saṃdhi-bandhana-karmaṇī ।।

ṣo-ḍaśaitāḥ parityajet
jihvāyāṃ hanu-vat tāsām adho dve rasa-bodhane ।
dve ca vācaḥ-pravartinyau nāsāyāṃ catur-uttarā ।।

viṃśatir gandha-vedinyau tāsām ekāṃ ca tālu-gām ।
ṣaṭ-pañcāśan nayanayor nimeṣonmeṣa-karmaṇī ।।

dve dve apāṅgayor dve ca tāsāṃ ṣaḍ iti varjayet ।
nāsā-netrāśritāḥ ṣaṣṭir lalāṭe sthapanī-śritām ।।

tatraikāṃ dve tathāvartau catasraś ca kacānta-gāḥ ।
saptaivaṃ varjayet tāsāṃ karṇayoḥ ṣo-ḍaśātra tu ।।

dve śabda-bodhane śaṅkhau sirās tā eva cāśritāḥ ।
dve śaṅkha-saṃdhi-ge tāsāṃ mūrdhni dvā-daśa tatra tu ।।

ekaikāṃ pṛthag utkṣepa-sīmantādhipati-sthitām ।
ity a-vedhya-vibhāgārthaṃ pratyaṅgaṃ varṇitāḥ sirāḥ ।।

a-vedhyās tatra kārtsnyena dehe aṣṭā-navatis tathā ।
saṃkīrṇā grathitāḥ kṣudrā vakrāḥ saṃdhiṣu cāśritāḥ ।।

tāsāṃ śatānāṃ saptānāṃ pādo asraṃ vahate pṛthak ।
vāta-pitta-kaphair juṣṭaṃ śuddhaṃ caivaṃ sthitā malāḥ ।।

śarīram anugṛhṇanti pīḍayanty anya-thā punaḥ ।
tatra śyāvāruṇāḥ sūkṣmāḥ pūrṇa-riktāḥ kṣaṇāt sirāḥ ।।

praspandinyaś ca vātāsraṃ vahante pitta-śoṇitam ।
sparśoṣṇāḥ śīghra-vāhinyo nīla-pītāḥ kaphaṃ punaḥ ।।

gauryaḥ snigdhāḥ sthirāḥ śītāḥ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ liṅga-saṃkare ।
gūḍhāḥ sama-sthitāḥ snigdhā rohiṇyaḥ śuddha-śoṇitam ।।

dhamanyo nābhi-saṃbaddhā viṃśatiś catur-uttarā ।
tābhiḥ parivṛtā nābhiś cakra-nābhir ivārakaiḥ ।।

ābhiḥ parivṛto nābhiś
tābhiś cordhvam adhas tiryag deho ayam anugṛhyate ।
srotāṃsi nāsike karṇau netre pāyv-āsya-mehanam ।।

stanau rakta-pathaś ceti nārīṇām adhikaṃ trayam ।
jīvitāyatanāny antaḥ srotāṃsy āhus trayo-daśa ।।

prāṇa-dhātu-malāmbho-'nna-vāhīny a-hita-sevanāt ।
tāni duṣṭāni rogāya viśuddhāni sukhāya ca ।।

sva-dhātu-sama-varṇāni vṛtta-sthūlāny aṇūni ca ।
srotāṃsi dīrghāṇy ākṛtyā pratāna-sadṛśāni ca ।।

āhāraś ca vihāraś ca yaḥ syād doṣa-guṇaiḥ samaḥ ।
dhātubhir vi-guṇo yaś ca srotasāṃ sa pradūṣakaḥ ।।

ati-pravṛttiḥ saṅgo vā sirāṇāṃ granthayo api vā ।
vi-mārgato vā gamanaṃ srotasāṃ duṣṭi-lakṣaṇam ।।

rotasāṃ duṣṭa-lakṣaṇam
bisānām iva sūkṣmāṇi dūraṃ pravisṛtāni ca ।
dvārāṇi srotasāṃ dehe raso yair upacīyate ।।

vyadhe tu srotasāṃ moha-kampādhmāna-vami-jvarāḥ ।
pralāpa-śūla-viṇ-mūtra-rodhā maraṇam eva vā ।।

sroto-viddham ato vaidyaḥ pratyākhyāya prasādhayet ।
uddhṛtya śalyaṃ yatnena sadyaḥ-kṣata-vidhānataḥ ।।

annasya paktā pittaṃ tu pācakākhyaṃ pureritam ।
doṣa-dhātu-malādīnām ūṣmety ātreya-śāsanam ।।

vāma-pārśvāśritaṃ nābheḥ kiñ-cit sūryasya maṇḍalam ।
tan-madhye maṇḍalaṃ saumyaṃ tan-madhye agnir vyavasthitaḥ ।।
jarāyu-mātra-pracchannaḥ kāca-kośa-stha-dīpa-vat ।।
tad-adhiṣṭhānam annasya grahaṇād grahaṇī matā ।
saiva dhanvantari-mate kalā pitta-dharāhvayā ।।

āyur-ārogya-vīryaujo-bhūta-dhātv-agni-puṣṭaye ।
sthitā pakvāśaya-dvāri bhukta-mārgārgaleva sā ।।

hukta-mārgārgaleva yā
bhuktam āmāśaye ruddhvā sā vipācya nayaty adhaḥ ।
bala-vaty a-balā tv annam āmam eva vimuñcati ।।

grahaṇyā balam agnir hi sa cāpi grahaṇī-balaḥ ।
dūṣite agnāv ato duṣṭā grahaṇī roga-kāriṇī ।।

yad annaṃ deha-dhātv-ojo-bala-varṇādi-poṣaṇam ।
tatrāgnir hetur āhārān na hy a-pakvād rasādayaḥ ।।

annaṃ kāle abhyavahṛtaṃ koṣṭhaṃ prāṇānilāhṛtam ।
dravair vibhinna-saṃghātaṃ nītaṃ snehena mārdavam ।।

oṣṭhe prāṇānilāhṛtam
saṃdhukṣitaḥ samānena pacaty āmāśaya-sthitam ।
audaryo agnir yathā bāhyaḥ sthālī-sthaṃ toya-taṇḍulam ।।

ādau ṣaḍ-rasam apy annaṃ madhurī-bhūtam īrayet ।
phenī-bhūtaṃ kaphaṃ yātaṃ vidāhād amla-tāṃ tataḥ ।।

hena-bhūtaṃ kaphaṃ yātaṃ
pittam āmāśayāt kuryāc cyavamānaṃ cyutaṃ punaḥ ।
agninā śoṣitaṃ pakvaṃ piṇḍitaṃ kaṭu mārutam ।।

bhaumāpyāgneya-vāyavyāḥ pañcoṣmāṇaḥ sa-nābhasāḥ ।
pañcāhāra-guṇān svān svān pārthivādīn pacanty anu ।।

yathā-svaṃ te ca puṣṇanti pakvā bhūta-guṇān pṛthak ।
pārthivāḥ pārthivān eva śeṣāḥ śeṣāṃś ca deha-gān ।।

athā-svaṃ te ca puṣyanti
kiṭṭaṃ sāraś ca tat pakvam annaṃ saṃbhavati dvi-dhā ।
tatrācchaṃ kiṭṭam annasya mūtraṃ vidyād ghanam śakṛt ।।

iṭṭaṃ sāras tathā pakvam
sāras tu saptabhir bhūyo yathā-svaṃ pacyate agnibhiḥ ।
rasād raktaṃ tato māṃsaṃ māṃsān medas tato asthi ca ।।

āṃsān medo asthi medasaḥ
asthno majjā tataḥ śukraṃ śukrād garbhaḥ prajāyate ।
kaphaḥ pittaṃ malāḥ kheṣu prasvedo nakha-roma ca ।।

aphaḥ pittaṃ malaḥ kheṣu
sneho akṣi-tvag-viṣām ojo dhātūnāṃ krama-śo malāḥ ।
prasāda-kiṭṭau dhātūnāṃ pākād evaṃ dvi-dharcchataḥ ।।

paras-paropasaṃstambhād dhātu-sneha-param-parā ।
ke-cid āhur aho-rātrāt ṣaḍ-ahād apare pare ।।

māsena yāti śukra-tvam annaṃ pāka-kramādibhiḥ ।
saṃtatā bhojya-dhātūnāṃ parivṛttis tu cakra-vat ।।

vṛṣyādīni prabhāveṇa sadyaḥ śukrādi kurvate ।
prāyaḥ karoty aho-rātrāt karmānyad api bheṣajam ।।

adyaḥ śukraṃ prakurvate
vyānena rasa-dhātur hi vikṣepocita-karmaṇā ।
yuga-pat sarvato ajasraṃ dehe vikṣipyate sadā ।।

kṣipyamāṇaḥ kha-vaiguṇyād rasaḥ sajjati yatra saḥ ।
tasmin vikāraṃ kurute khe varṣam iva toya-daḥ ।।

doṣāṇām api caivaṃ syād eka-deśa-prakopaṇam ।
anna-bhautika-dhātv-agni-karmeti paribhāṣitam ।।

annasya paktā sarveṣāṃ paktṝṇām adhiko mataḥ ।
tan-mūlās te hi tad-vṛddhi-kṣaya-vṛddhi-kṣayātmakāḥ ।।

tasmāt taṃ vidhi-vad yuktair anna-pānendhanair hitaiḥ ।
pālayet prayatas tasya sthitau hy āyur-bala-sthitiḥ ।।

samaḥ samāne sthāna-sthe viṣamo agnir vi-mārga-ge ।
pittābhimūrchite tīkṣṇo mando asmin kapha-pīḍite ।।

samo agnir viṣamas tīkṣṇo mandaś caivaṃ catur-vidhaḥ ।
yaḥ pacet samyag evānnaṃ bhuktaṃ samyak samas tv asau ।।

huktaṃ samyak samas tu saḥ
viṣamo a-samyag apy āśu samyag vāpi cirāt pacet ।
tīkṣṇo vahniḥ pacec chīghram a-samyag api bhojanam ।।

iṣamo a-samyag evāśu amyag eva cirāt pacet
mandas tu samyag apy annam upayuktaṃ cirāt pacet ।
kṛtvāsya-śoṣāṭopāntra-kūjanādhmāna-gauravam ।।

pabhuktaṃ cirāt pacet
śānte agnau mriyate yukte ciraṃ jīvaty an-āmayaḥ ।
rogī syād vikṛte mūlam agni-stambhān nirucyate ।।

gni-stambhān nirūpyate
saha-jaṃ kāla-jaṃ yukti-kṛtaṃ deha-balaṃ tri-dhā ।
tatra sat-tva-śarīrotthaṃ prākṛtaṃ saha-jaṃ balam ।।

vayaḥ-kṛtam ṛtūtthaṃ ca kāla-jaṃ yukti-jaṃ punaḥ ।
vihārāhāra-janitaṃ tathorjas-kara-yoga-jam ।।

deśo alpa-vāri-dru-nago jāṅgalaḥ sv-alpa-roga-daḥ ।
ānūpo viparīto asmāt samaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

majja-medo-vasā-mūtra-pitta-śleṣma-śakṛnty asṛk ।
raso jalaṃ ca dehe asminn ekaikāñjali-vardhitam ।।

pṛthak sva-prasṛtaṃ proktam ojo-mastiṣka-retasām ।
dvāv añjalī tu stanyasya catvāro rajasaḥ striyāḥ ।।
sama-dhātor idaṃ mānaṃ vidyād vṛddhi-kṣayāv ataḥ ।।
śukrāsṛg-garbhiṇī-bhojya-ceṣṭā-garbhāśayartuṣu ।
yaḥ syād doṣo adhikas tena prakṛtiḥ sapta-dhoditā ।।

rakṛtiḥ sapta-dhā smṛtā
vibhu-tvād āśu-kāri-tvād bali-tvād anya-kopanāt ।
svātantryād bahu-roga-tvād doṣāṇāṃ prabalo anilaḥ ।।

prāyo ata eva pavanādhyuṣitā manuṣyā doṣātmakāḥ sphuṭita-dhūsara-keśa-gātrāḥ ।
śīta-dviṣaś cala-dhṛti-smṛti-buddhi-ceṣṭā-sauhārda-dṛṣṭi-gatayo ati-bahu-pralāpāḥ ।।

alpa-vitta-bala-jīvita-nidrāḥ sanna-sakta-cala-jarjara-vācaḥ ।
nāstikā bahu-bhujaḥ sa-vilāsā gīta-hāsa-mṛgayā-kali-lolāḥ ।।

lpa-pitta-kapha-jīvita-nidrāḥ lpa-vitta-kapha-jīvita-nidrāḥ 
lpa-pitta-bala-jīvita-nidrāḥ
madhurāmla-paṭūṣṇa-sātmya-kāṅkṣāḥ kṛśa-dīrghākṛtayaḥ sa-śabda-yātāḥ ।
na dṛḍhā na jitendriyā na cāryā na ca kāntā-dayitā bahu-prajā vā ।।

ṛśa-dīrghākṛtayaḥ sa-śabda-yānāḥ
netrāṇi caiṣāṃ khara-dhūsarāṇi vṛttāny a-cārūṇi mṛtopamāni ।
unmīlitānīva bhavanti supte śaila-drumāṃs te gaganaṃ ca yānti ।।

etrāṇi vaiṣāṃ khara-dhūsarāṇi
a-dhanyā matsarādhmātāḥ stenāḥ prodbaddha-piṇḍikāḥ ।
śva-śṛgāloṣṭra-gṛdhrākhu-kākānūkāś ca vātikāḥ ।।

tenāḥ prodvṛtta-piṇḍikāḥ
pittaṃ vahnir vahni-jaṃ vā yad asmāt pittodriktas tīkṣṇa-tṛṣṇā-bubhukṣaḥ ।
gauroṣṇāṅgas tāmra-hastāṅghri-vaktraḥ śūro mānī piṅga-keśo alpa-romā ।।

ittodriktas tīvra-tṛṣṇā-bubhukṣaḥ
dayita-mālya-vilepana-maṇḍanaḥ su-caritaḥ śucir āśrita-vatsalaḥ ।
vibhava-sāhasa-buddhi-balānvito bhavati bhīṣu gatir dviṣatām api ।।

medhāvī pra-śithila-saṃdhi-bandha-māṃso nārīṇām an-abhimato alpa-śukra-kāmaḥ ।
āvāsaḥ palita-taraṅga-nīlikānāṃ bhuṅkte annaṃ madhura-kaṣāya-tikta-śītam ।।

gharma-dveṣī svedanaḥ pūti-gandhir bhūry-uccāra-krodha-pānāśanerṣyaḥ ।
suptaḥ paśyet karṇikārān palāśān dig-dāholkā-vidyud-arkānalāṃś ca ।।

tanūni piṅgāni calāni caiṣāṃ tanv-alpa-pakṣmāṇi hima-priyāṇi ।
krodhena madyena raveś ca bhāsā rāgaṃ vrajanty āśu vilocanāni ।।

anūni piṅgāni calāni vaiṣāṃ
madhyāyuṣo madhya-balāḥ piṇḍitāḥ kleśa-bhīravaḥ ।
vyāghrarkṣa-kapi-mārjāra-yakṣānūkāś ca paittikāḥ ।।

-vṛkānūkāś ca paittikāḥ
śleṣmā somaḥ śleṣmalas tena saumyo gūḍha-snigdha-śliṣṭa-saṃdhy-asthi-māṃsaḥ ।
kṣut-tṛḍ-duḥkha-kleśa-gharmair a-tapto buddhyā yuktaḥ sāttvikaḥ satya-saṃdhaḥ ।।

priyaṅgu-dūrvā-śara-kāṇḍa-śastra- go-rocanā-padma-suvarṇa-varṇaḥ ।
pralamba-bāhuḥ pṛthu-pīna-vakṣā mahā-lalāṭo ghana-nīla-keśaḥ ।।

mṛdv-aṅgaḥ sama-su-vibhakta-cāru-deho bahv-ojo-rati-rasa-śukra-putra-bhṛtyaḥ ।
dharmātmā vadati na niṣṭhuraṃ ca jātu pracchannaṃ vahati dṛḍhaṃ ciraṃ ca vairam ।। 

।।

ṛdv-aṅgaḥ sama-su-vibhakta-cāru-varṣmā
sa-mada-dvi-radendra-tulya-yāto jala-dāmbho-dhi-mṛdaṅga-siṃha-ghoṣaḥ ।
smṛti-mān abhiyoga-vān vinīto na ca bālye apy ati-rodano na lolaḥ ।।

ala-dāmbho-dhi-mṛdaṅga-śaṅkha-ghoṣaḥ
tiktaṃ kaṣāyaṃ kaṭukoṣṇa-rūkṣam alpaṃ sa bhuṅkte bala-vāṃs tathāpi ।
raktānta-su-snigdha-viśāla-dīrgha- su-vyakta-śuklāsita-pakṣmalākṣaḥ ।।

alpa-vyāhāra-krodha-pānāśanehaḥ prājyāyur-vitto dīrgha-darśī vadānyaḥ ।
śrāddho gambhīraḥ sthūla-lakṣaḥ kṣamā-vān āryo nidrālur dīrgha-sūtraḥ kṛta-jñaḥ ।। 

।।

lpa-vyāhāra-krodha-pānāśanerṣyaḥ rājyāyur-vṛtto dīrgha-darśī vadānyaḥ śrāddho gambhīraḥ sthūla-lakṣyaḥ kṣamā-vān āryo nidrālur 
dīrgha-sūtrī kṛta-jñaḥ
ṛjur vipaścit su-bhagaḥ su-lajjo bhakto gurūṇāṃ sthira-sauhṛdaś ca ।
svapne sa-padmān sa-vihaṅga-mālāṃs toyāśayān paśyati toya-dāṃś ca ।।

ṛjur vipaścit su-bhagaḥ sa-lajjo
brahma-rudrendra-varuṇa-tārkṣya-haṃsa-gajādhipaiḥ ।
śleṣma-prakṛtayas tulyās tathā siṃhāśva-go-vṛṣaiḥ ।।

prakṛtīr dvaya-sarvotthā dvandva-sarva-guṇodaye ।
śaucāstikyādibhiś caivaṃ guṇair guṇa-mayīr vadet ।।

vayas tv ā-ṣo-ḍaśād bālaṃ tatra dhātv-indriyaujasām ।
vṛddhir ā-saptater madhyaṃ tatrā-vṛddhiḥ paraṃ kṣayaḥ ।।

svaṃ svaṃ hasta-trayaṃ sārdhaṃ vapuḥ pātraṃ sukhāyuṣoḥ ।
na ca yad yuktam udriktair aṣṭābhir ninditair nijaiḥ ।।

a-romaśāsita-sthūla-dīrgha-tvaiḥ sa-viparyayaiḥ ।
su-snigdhā mṛdavaḥ sūkṣmā naika-mūlāḥ sthirāḥ kacāḥ ।।

lalāṭam unnataṃ śliṣṭa-śaṅkham ardhendu-saṃnibham ।
karṇau nīconnatau paścān mahāntau śliṣṭa-māṃsalau ।।

netre vyaktāsita-site su-baddha-ghana-pakṣmaṇī ।
unnatāgrā mahocchvāsā pīnarjur nāsikā samā ।।

u-baddhe ghana-pakṣmaṇī
oṣṭhau raktāv an-udvṛttau mahatyau nolbaṇe hanū ।
mahad āsyaṃ ghanā dantāḥ snigdhāḥ ślakṣṇāḥ sitāḥ samāḥ ।।

jihvā raktāyatā tanvī māṃsalaṃ cibukaṃ mahat ।
grīvā hrasvā ghanā vṛttā skandhāv unnata-pīvarau ।।

udaraṃ dakṣiṇāvarta-gūḍha-nābhi samunnatam ।
tanu-raktonnata-nakhaṃ snigdhaṃ ā-tāmra-māṃsalam ।।

dīrghā-cchidrāṅguli mahat pāṇi-pādaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
gūḍha-vaṃśaṃ bṛhat pṛṣṭhaṃ nigūḍhāḥ saṃdhayo dṛḍhāḥ ।।

ūḍha-vaṃśaṃ mahat pṛṣṭhaṃ
dhīraḥ svaro anunādī ca varṇaḥ snigdhaḥ sthira-prabhaḥ ।
sva-bhāva-jaṃ sthiraṃ sat-tvam a-vikāri vipatsv api ।।

uttarottara-su-kṣetraṃ vapur garbhādi-nī-rujam ।
āyāma-jñāna-vijñānair vardhamānaṃ śanaiḥ śubham ।।

iti sarva-guṇopete śarīre śaradāṃ śatam ।
āyur aiśvaryam iṣṭāś ca sarve bhāvāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।

tvag-raktādīni sat-tvāntāny agryāṇy aṣṭau yathottaram ।
bala-pramāṇa-jñānārthaṃ sārāṇy uktāni dehinām ।।

grāṇy aṣṭau yathottaram
sārair upetaḥ sarvaiḥ syāt paraṃ gaurava-saṃyutaḥ ।
sarvārambheṣu cāśā-vān sahiṣṇuḥ san-matiḥ sthiraḥ ।।

ahiṣṇuḥ su-matiḥ sthiraḥ
an-utsekaṃ a-dainyaṃ ca sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca sevate ।
sat-tva-vāṃs tapyamānas tu rājaso naiva tāmasaḥ ।।

at-tva-vān stabhyamānas tu
dāna-śīla-dayā-satya-brahma-carya-kṛta-jña-tāḥ ।
rasāyanāni maitrī ca puṇyāyur-vṛddhi-kṛd gaṇaḥ ।।

”ārīrasthāna
saptottaraṃ marma-śataṃ teṣām ekā-daśādiśet ।
pṛthak sakthnos tathā bāhvos trīṇi koṣṭhe navorasi ।।

pṛṣṭhe catur-daśordhvaṃ tu jatros triṃśac ca sapta ca ।
madhye pāda-talasyāhur abhito madhyamāṅgulīm ।।

tala-hṛn nāma rujayā tatra viddhasya pañca-tā ।
aṅguṣṭhāṅguli-madhya-sthaṃ kṣipraṃ ākṣepa-māraṇam ।।

tasyordhvaṃ dvy-aṅgule kūrcaḥ pāda-bhramaṇa-kampa-kṛt ।
gulpha-saṃdher adhaḥ kūrca-śiraḥ śopha-rujā-karam ।।

jaṅghā-caraṇayoḥ saṃdhau gulpho ruk-stambha-māndya-kṛt ।
jaṅghāntare tv indra-vastir mārayaty asṛjaḥ kṣayāt ।।

ulpho ruk-stambha-ṣāṇḍhya-kṛt ulpho ruk-stambha-khāñjya-kṛt 
ulpho ruk-stambha-jāḍya-kṛt
jaṅghorvoḥ saṃgame jānu khañja-tā tatra jīvataḥ ।
jānunas try-aṅgulād ūrdhvam āṇy-ūru-stambha-śopha-kṛt ।।

urvy ūru-madhye tad-vedhāt sakthi-śoṣo asra-saṃkṣayāt ।
ūru-mūle lohitākṣaṃ hanti pakṣam asṛk-kṣayāt ।।

ūru-mūle lohitākhyaṃ
muṣka-vaṅkṣaṇayor madhye viṭapaṃ ṣaṇḍha-tā-karam ।
iti sakthnos tathā bāhvor maṇi-bandho atra gulpha-vat ।।

iṭipaṃ ṣaṇḍha-tā-karam
kūrparaṃ jānu-vat kauṇyaṃ tayor viṭapa-vat punaḥ ।
kakṣākṣa-madhye kakṣā-dhṛk kuṇi-tvaṃ tatra jāyate ।।

sthūlāntra-baddhaḥ sadyo-ghno viḍ-vāta-vamano gudaḥ ।
mūtrāśayo dhanur-vakro vastir alpāsra-māṃsa-gaḥ ।।

ekādho-vadano madhye kaṭyāḥ sadyo nihanty asūn ।
ṛte aśmarī-vraṇād viddhas tatrāpy ubhayataś ca saḥ ।।

atrāpy ubhayataś ca yaḥ
mūtra-srāvy ekato bhinne vraṇo rohec ca yatnataḥ ।
dehāma-pakva-sthānānāṃ madhye sarva-sirāśrayaḥ ।।

nābhiḥ so api hi sadyo-ghno dvāram āmāśayasya ca ।
sat-tvādi-dhāma hṛdayaṃ stanoraḥ-koṣṭha-madhya-gam ।।

stana-rohita-mūlākhye dvy-aṅgule stanayor vadet ।
ūrdhvādho asra-kaphāpūrṇa-koṣṭho naśyet tayoḥ kramāt ।।

ūrdhvādho asṛk-kaphāpūrṇa-
apastambhāv uraḥ-pārśve nāḍyāv anila-vāhinī ।
raktena pūrṇa-koṣṭho atra śvāsāt kāsāc ca naśyati ।।

aktasya pūrṇa-koṣṭho atra
pṛṣṭha-vaṃśorasor madhye tayor eva ca pārśvayoḥ ।
adho aṃsa-kūṭayor vidyād apālāpākhya-marmaṇī ।।

tayoḥ koṣṭhe asṛjā pūrṇe naśyed yātena pūya-tām ।
pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭha-vaṃśasya śroṇi-karṇau prati sthite ।।

śroṇi-karṇa-pratiṣṭhite śroṇi-karṇau pratiṣṭhitau
vaṃśāśrite sphijor ūrdhvaṃ kaṭīka-taruṇe smṛte ।
tatra rakta-kṣayāt pāṇdur hīna-rūpo vinaśyati ।।

pṛṣṭha-vaṃśaṃ hy ubhayato yau saṃdhī kaṭi-pārśvayoḥ ।
jaghanasya bahir-bhāge marmaṇī tau kukundarau ।।

ṛṣṭha-vaṃśasyobhayato
ceṣṭā-hānir adhaḥ-kāye sparśā-jñānaṃ ca tad-vyadhāt ।
pārśvāntara-nibaddhau yāv upari śroṇi-karṇayoḥ ।।

āśaya-cchādanau tau tu nitambau taruṇāsthi-gau ।
adhaḥ-śarīre śopho atra daurbalyaṃ maraṇaṃ tataḥ ।।

āśayācchādanau tau tu
pārśvāntara-nibaddhau ca madhye jaghana-pārśvayoḥ ।
tiryag ūrdhvaṃ ca nirdiṣṭau pārśva-saṃdhī tayor vyadhāt ।।

adhyau jaghana-pārśvayoḥ irdiṣṭau pārśva-saṃdhī tau 
iryag ūrdhvaṃ tayor vyadhāt
rakta-pūrita-koṣṭhasya śarīrāntara-saṃbhavaḥ ।
stana-mūlārjave bhāge pṛṣṭha-vaṃśāśraye sire ।।

bṛhatyau tatra viddhasya maraṇaṃ rakta-saṃkṣayāt ।
bāhu-mūlābhisaṃbaddhe pṛṣṭha-vaṃśasya pārśvayoḥ ।।

aṃsayoḥ phalake bāhu-svāpa-śoṣau tayor vyadhāt ।
grīvām ubhayataḥ snāvnī grīvā-bāhu-śiro-'ntare ।।

-svāpa-śoṣau tayor vyadhe -svāpa-śophau tayor vyadhe 
-svāpa-śophau tayor vyadhāt
skandhāṃsa-pīṭha-saṃbandhāv aṃsau bāhu-kriyā-harau ।
kaṇṭha-nālīm ubhayataḥ sirā hanu-samāśritāḥ ।।

kandhāṃsa-pīṭha-baddhārthāv kandhāṃsa-pīṭha-bandhārthāv 
kandhāṃsa-pīṭha-saṃbaddhāv
catasras tāsu nīle dve manye dve marmaṇī smṛte ।
svara-praṇāśa-vaikṛtyaṃ rasā-jñānaṃ ca tad-vyadhe ।।

vara-praṇāśa-vaikṛtya- vara-praṇāśo vaikṛtyaṃ 
-rasā-jñānaṃ ca tad-vyadhe
kaṇṭha-nālīm ubhayato jihvā-nāsā-gatāḥ sirāḥ ।
pṛthak catasras tāḥ sadyo ghnanty asūn mātṛkāhvayāḥ ।।

kṛkāṭike śiro-grīvā-saṃdhau tatra calaṃ śiraḥ ।
adhas-tāt karṇayor nimne vidhure śruti-hāriṇī ।।

-saṃdhī tatra calaṃ śiraḥ
phaṇāv ubhayato ghrāṇa-mārgaṃ śrotra-pathānugau ।
antar-gala-sthitau vedhād gandha-vijñāna-hāriṇau ।।

netrayor bāhyato apāṅgau bhruvoḥ pucchāntayor adhaḥ ।
tathopari bhruvor nimnāv āvartāv āndhyam eṣu tu ।।

anu-karṇaṃ lalāṭānte śaṅkhau sadyo-vināśanau ।
keśānte śaṅkhayor ūrdhvam utkṣepau sthapani punaḥ ।।

bhruvor madhye traye apy atra śalye jīved an-uddhṛte ।
svayaṃ vā patite pākāt sadyo naśyati tūddhṛte ।।

jihvākṣi-nāsikā-śrotra-kha-catuṣṭaya-saṃgame ।
tālūny āsyāni catvāri srotasāṃ teṣu marmasu ।।

viddhaḥ śṛṅgāṭakākhyeṣu sadyas tyajati jīvitam ।
kapāle saṃdhayaḥ pañca sīmantās tiryag-ūrdhva-gāḥ ।।

apāla-saṃdhayaḥ pañca
bhramonmāda-mano-nāśais teṣu viddheṣu naśyati ।
āntaro mastakasyordhvaṃ sirā-saṃdhi-samāgamaḥ ।।

ntare mastakasyordhvaṃ
romāvarto adhipo nāma marma sadyo haraty asūn ।
viṣamaṃ spandanaṃ yatra pīḍite ruk ca marma tat ।।

māṃsāsthi-snāyu-dhamanī-sirā-saṃdhi-samāgamaḥ ।
syān marmeti ca tenātra su-tarāṃ jīvitaṃ sthitam ।।

bāhulyena tu nirdeśaḥ ṣo-ḍhaivaṃ marma-kalpanā ।
prāṇāyatana-sāmānyād aikyaṃ vā marmaṇāṃ matam ।।

ikyaṃ vā marmaṇāṃ smṛtam
māṃsa-jāni daśendrākhya-tala-hṛt-stana-rohitāḥ ।
śaṅkhau kaṭīka-taruṇe nitambāv aṃsayoḥ phale ।।

asthny aṣṭau snāva-marmāṇi trayo-viṃśatir āṇayaḥ ।
kūrca-kūrca-śiro-'pāṅga-kṣiprotkṣepāṃsa-vastayaḥ ।।

sthny aṣṭau snāyu-marmāṇi
gudāpastambha-vidhura-śṛṅgāṭāni navādiśet ।
marmāṇi dhamanī-sthāni sapta-triṃśat sirāśrayāḥ ।।

udo apastambha-vidhura-
bṛhatyau mātṛkā nīle manye kakṣā-dharau phaṇau ।
viṭape hṛdayaṃ nābhiḥ pārśva-saṃdhī stanādhare ।।

ārśva-saṃdhī stanāntare
apālāpau sthapany urvyaś catasro lohitāni ca ।
saṃdhau viṃśatir āvartau maṇi-bandhau kukundarau ।।

sīmantāḥ kūrparau gulphau kṛkāṭyau jānunī patiḥ ।
māṃsa-marma gudo anyeṣāṃ snāvni kakṣā-dharau tathā ।।

nāvnī kakṣā-dharau tathā
viṭapau vidhurākhye ca śṛṅgāṭāni sirāsu tu ।
apastambhāv apāṅgau ca dhamanī-sthaṃ na taiḥ smṛtam ।।

viddhe ajasram asṛk-srāvo māṃsa-dhāvana-vat tanuḥ ।
pāṇḍu-tvam indriyā-jñānaṃ maraṇam cāśu māṃsa-je ।।

araṇam vāśu māṃsa-je
majjānvito accho vicchinnaḥ srāvo ruk cāsthi-marmaṇi ।
āyāmākṣepaka-stambhāḥ snāva-je abhyadhikaṃ rujā ।।

nāva-je abhyadhikaṃ rujaḥ nāva-je abhyadhikā rujaḥ 
snāyu-ge abhyadhikaṃ rujā
yāna-sthānāsanā-śaktir vaikalyam atha vāntakaḥ ।
raktaṃ sa-śabda-phenoṣṇaṃ dhamanī-sthe vi-cetasaḥ ।।

sirā-marma-vyadhe sāndram ajasraṃ bahv asṛk sravet ।
tat-kṣayāt tṛḍ-bhrama-śvāsa-moha-hidhmābhir antakaḥ ।।

vastu śūkair ivākīrṇaṃ rūḍhe ca kuṇi-khañja-tā ।
bala-ceṣṭā-kṣayaḥ śoṣaḥ parva-śophaś ca saṃdhi-je ।।

nābhi-śaṅkhādhipāpāna-hṛc-chṛṅgāṭaka-vastayaḥ ।
aṣṭau ca mātṛkāḥ sadyo nighnanty ekān-na-viṃśatiḥ ।।

ighnanty ekona-viṃśatiḥ
saptāhaḥ paramas teṣāṃ kālaḥ kālasya karṣaṇe ।
trayas-triṃśad-apastambha-tala-hṛt-pārśva-saṃdhayaḥ ।।

aptāhaḥ paramaṃ teṣāṃ
kaṭī-taruṇa-sīmanta-stana-mūlendra-vastayaḥ ।
kṣiprāpālāpa-bṛhatī-nitamba-stana-rohitāḥ ।।

kālāntara-prāṇa-harā māsa-māsārdha-jīvitāḥ ।
utkṣepau sthapanī trīṇi vi-śalya-ghnāni tatra hi ।।

i-śalya-ghnāni tatra tu
vāyur māṃsa-vasā-majja-mastuluṅgāni śoṣayet ।
śalyāpāye vinirgacchan śvāsāt kāsāc ca hanty asūn ।।

phaṇāv apāṅgau vidhure nīle manye kṛkāṭike ।
aṃsāṃsa-phalakāvarta-viṭaporvī-kukundarāḥ ।।

haṇāv apāṅgau vidhurau
sa-jānu-lohitākṣāṇi-kakṣā-dhṛk-kūrca-kūrparāḥ ।
vaikalyam iti catvāri catvāriṃśac ca kurvate ।।

a-jānu-lohitākhyāni-
haranti tāny api prāṇān kadā-cid abhighātataḥ ।
aṣṭau kūrca-śiro-gulpha-maṇi-bandhā rujā-karāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ viṭapa-kakṣā-dhṛg-urvyaḥ kūrca-śirāṃsi ca ।
dvā-daśāṅgula-mānāni dvy-aṅgule maṇi-bandhane ।।

-urvī-kūrca-śirāṃsi ca
gulphau ca stana-mūle ca try-aṅgulaṃ jānu-kūrparam ।
apāna-vasti-hṛn-nābhi-nīlāḥ sīmanta-mātṛkāḥ ।।

ry-aṅgulau jānu-kūrparau -nīlā-sīmanta-mātṛkāḥ
kūrca-śṛṅgāṭa-manyāś ca triṃśad ekena varjitāḥ ।
ātma-pāṇi-talonmānāḥ śeṣāṇy ardhāṅgulaṃ vadet ।।

pañcāśat ṣaṭ ca marmāṇi tila-vrīhi-samāny api ।
iṣṭāni marmāṇy anyeṣāṃ catur-dhoktāḥ sirās tu yāḥ ।।

tarpayanti vapuḥ kṛtsnaṃ tā marmāṇy āśritās tataḥ ।
tat-kṣatāt kṣata-jāty-artha-pravṛtter dhātu-saṃkṣaye ।।

at-kṣatāt kṣata-jāty-arthaṃ ravṛttir dhātu-saṃkṣaye
vṛddhaś calo rujas tīvrāḥ pratanoti samīrayan ।
tejas tad uddhṛtaṃ dhatte tṛṣṇā-śoṣa-mada-bhramān ।।

svinna-srasta-ślatha-tanuṃ haraty enaṃ tato antakaḥ ।
vardhayet saṃdhito gātraṃ marmaṇy abhihate drutam ।।

chedanāt saṃdhi-deśasya saṃkucanti sirā hy ataḥ ।
jīvitaṃ prāṇināṃ tatra rakte tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhati ।।

su-vikṣato apy ato jīved a-marmaṇi na marmaṇi ।
prāṇa-ghātini jīvet tu kaś-cid vaidya-guṇena cet ।।

a-samagrābhighātāc ca so api vaikalyam aśnute ।
tasmāt kṣāra-viṣāgny-ādīn yatnān marmasu varjayet ।।

marmābhighātaḥ sv-alpo api prāya-śo bādhate-tarām ।
rogā marmāśrayās tad-vat prakrāntā yatnato api ca ।।

ogā marmāśritās tad-vat

”ārīrasthāna
puṣpaṃ phalasya dhūmo agner varṣasya jala-dodayaḥ ।
yathā bhaviṣyato liṅgaṃ riṣṭaṃ mṛtyos tathā dhruvam ।।

āyuṣ-mati kriyāḥ sarvāḥ sa-phalāḥ saṃprayojitāḥ ।
bhavanti bhiṣajāṃ bhūtyai kṛta-jña iva bhū-bhuji ।।

kṣīṇāyuṣi kṛtaṃ karma vyarthaṃ kṛtam ivādhame ।
a-yaśo deha-saṃdehaṃ svārtha-hāniṃ ca yacchati ।।

āyāsād deha-saṃdehaṃ
tarhīdānīṃ gatāsūnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ saṃpracakṣate ।
vikṛtiḥ prakṛteḥ prājñaiḥ pradiṣṭā riṣṭa-saṃjñayā ।।

tad idānīṃ gatāsūnāṃ
ariṣṭaṃ nāsti maraṇaṃ dṛṣṭa-riṣṭaṃ ca jīvitam ।
ariṣṭe riṣṭa-vijñānaṃ na ca riṣṭe apy a-naipuṇāt ।।

ke-cit tu tad dvi-dhety āhuḥ sthāyy-a-sthāyi-vibhedataḥ ।
doṣāṇām api bāhulyād riṣṭābhāsaḥ samudbhavet ।।

sa doṣāṇāṃ śame śāmyet sthāyy avaśyaṃ tu mṛtyave ।
rūpendriya-svara-cchāyā-praticchāyā-kriyādiṣu ।।

ad doṣāṇāṃ śame śāmyet
anyeṣv api ca bhāveṣu prākṛteṣv a-nimittataḥ ।
vikṛtir yā samāsena riṣṭaṃ tad iti lakṣayet ।।

keśa-roma-nir-abhyaṅgaṃ yasyābhyaktam ivekṣyate ।
yasyāty-arthaṃ cale netre stabdhāntar-gata-nirgate ।।

jihme vistṛta-saṃkṣipte saṃkṣipta-vinata-bhruṇī ।
udbhrānta-darśane hīna-darśane nakulopame ।।

kapotābhe alātābhe srute lulita-pakṣmaṇī ।
nāsikāty-artha-vivṛtā saṃvṛtā piṭikācitā ।।

ucchūnā sphuṭitā mlānā yasyauṣṭho yāty adho adharaḥ ।
ūrdhvaṃ dvitīyaḥ syātāṃ vā pakva-jambū-nibhāv ubhau ।।

dantāḥ sa-śarkarāḥ śyāvās tāmrāḥ puṣpita-paṅkitāḥ ।
sahasaiva pateyur vā jihvā jihmā visarpiṇī ।।

śūnā śuṣkā guruḥ śyāvā liptā suptā sa-kaṇṭakā ।
śiraḥ śiro-dharā voḍhuṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ vā bhāram ātmanaḥ ।।

hanū vā piṇḍam āsya-sthaṃ śaknuvanti na yasya ca ।
yasyā-nimittam aṅgāni gurūṇy ati-laghūni vā ।।

viṣa-doṣād vinā yasya khebhyo raktaṃ pravartate ।
utsiktaṃ mehanaṃ yasya vṛṣaṇāv ati-niḥsṛtau ।।

ato anya-thā vā yasya syāt sarve te kāla-coditāḥ ।
yasyā-pūrvāḥ sirā-lekhā bālendv-ākṛtayo api vā ।।

arve te kāla-noditāḥ
lalāṭe vasti-śīrṣe vā ṣaṇ māsān na sa jīvati ।
padminī-pattra-vat toyaṃ śarīre yasya dehinaḥ ।।

plavate plavamānasya ṣaṇ māsās tasya jīvitam ।
haritābhāḥ sirā yasya roma-kūpāś ca saṃvṛtāḥ ।।

ṣaṇ-māsaṃ tasya jīvitam ṣaṇ-māsāt tasya jīvitam ṣaṇ 
māsāṃs tasya jīvitam
so amlābhilāṣī puruṣaḥ pittān maraṇam aśnute ।
yasya go-maya-cūrṇābhaṃ cūrṇaṃ mūrdhni mukhe api vā ।।

sa-snehaṃ mūrdhni dhūmo vā māsāntaṃ tasya jīvitam ।
mūrdhni bhruvor vā kurvanti sīmantāvartakā navāḥ ।।

ūrdhni bhruvor vā yasya syuḥ
mṛtyuṃ svasthasya ṣaḍ-rātrāt tri-rātrād āturasya tu ।
jihvā śyāvā mukhaṃ pūti savyam akṣi nimajjati ।।

ri-rātrād āturasya ca
khagā vā mūrdhni līyante yasya taṃ parivarjayet ।
yasya snātānuliptasya pūrvaṃ śuṣyaty uro bhṛśam ।।

ārdreṣu sarva-gātreṣu so ardha-māsaṃ na jīvati ।
a-kasmād yuga-pad gātre varṇau prākṛta-vaikṛtau ।।

tathaivopacaya-glāni-raukṣya-snehādi mṛtyave ।
yasya sphuṭeyur aṅgulyo nākṛṣṭā na sa jīvati ।।

kṣava-kāsādiṣu tathā yasyā-pūrvo dhvanir bhavet ।
hrasvo dīrgho ati vocchvāsaḥ pūtiḥ surabhir eva vā ।।

āplutān-āplute kāye yasya gandho ati-mānuṣaḥ ।
mala-vastra-vraṇādau vā varṣāntaṃ tasya jīvitam ।।

ala-vastra-vraṇādye vā
bhajante aty-aṅga-saurasyād yaṃ yūkā-makṣikādayaḥ ।
tyajanti vāti-vairasyāt so api varṣaṃ na jīvati ।।

satatoṣmasu gātreṣu śaityaṃ yasyopalakṣyate ।
śīteṣu bhṛśam auṣṇyaṃ vā svedaḥ stambho apy a-hetukaḥ ।।

vedaḥ stambho aty a-hetukaḥ
yo jāta-śīta-piṭikaḥ śītāṅgo vā vidahyate ।
uṣṇa-dveṣī ca śitārtaḥ sa pretādhipa-go-caraḥ ।।

śītāṅgo vātidahyate śītāṅgo vāpi dahyate
urasy ūṣmā bhaved yasya jaṭhare cāti-śīta-tā ।
bhinnaṃ purīṣaṃ tṛṣṇā ca yathā pretas tathaiva saḥ ।।

aṭhare vāti-śīta-tā
mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ niṣṭhyūtaṃ śukraṃ vāpsu nimajjati ।
niṣṭhyūtaṃ bahu-varṇaṃ vā yasya māsāt sa naśyati ।।

ghanī-bhūtam ivākāśam ākāśam iva yo ghanam ।
a-mūrtam iva mūrtaṃ ca mūrtaṃ cā-mūrta-vat sthitam ।।
