tejasvy a-tejas tad-vac ca śuklaṃ kṛṣṇam a-sac ca sat ।
a-netra-rogaś candraṃ ca bahu-rūpam a-lāñchanam ।।

ejasy a-tejas tad-vac ca -netra-rogī candraṃ ca
jāgrad rakṣāṃsi gandharvān pretān anyāṃś ca tad-vidhān ।
rūpaṃ vy-ākṛti tat tac ca yaḥ paśyati sa naśyati ।।

ūpaṃ vy-ākṛti tad-vac ca
saptarṣīṇāṃ samīpa-sthāṃ yo na paśyaty arundhatīm ।
dhruvam ākāśa-gaṅgāṃ vā sa na paśyati tāṃ samām ।।

megha-toyaugha-nirghoṣa-vīṇā-paṇava-veṇu-jān ।
śṛṇoty anyāṃś ca yaḥ śabdān a-sato na sato api vā ।।

niṣpīḍya karṇau śṛṇuyān na yo dhukadhukā-svanam ।
tad-vad gandha-rasa-sparśān manyate yo viparyayāt ।।

a yo dhukadhuka-svanam
sarva-śo vā na yo yaś ca dīpa-gandhaṃ na jighrati ।
vidhinā yasya doṣāya svāsthyāyā-vidhinā rasāḥ ।।

yaḥ pāṃsuneva kīrṇāṅgo yo aṅge ghātaṃ na vetti vā ।
antareṇa tapas tīvraṃ yogaṃ vā vidhi-pūrvakam ।।

o bhasmaneva kīrṇāṅgo
jānāty atīndriyaṃ yaś ca teṣāṃ maraṇam ādiśet ।
hīno dīnaḥ svaro a-vyakto yasya syād gadgado api vā ।।

sahasā yo vimuhyed vā vivakṣur na sa jīvati ।
svarasya dur-balī-bhāvaṃ hāniṃ ca bala-varṇayoḥ ।।

roga-vṛddhim a-yuktyā ca dṛṣṭvā maraṇam ādiśet ।
apa-svaraṃ bhāṣamāṇaṃ prāptaṃ maraṇam ātmanaḥ ।।

śrotāraṃ cāsya śabdasya dūrataḥ parivarjayet ।
saṃsthānena pramāṇena varṇena prabhayāpi vā ।।

śrotāraṃ tasya śabdasya śrotāraṃ vāsya śabdasya
chāyā vivartate yasya svapne api preta eva saḥ ।
ātapādarśa-toyādau yā saṃsthāna-pramāṇataḥ ।।

chāyāṅgāt saṃbhavaty uktā praticchāyeti sā punaḥ ।
varṇa-prabhāśrayā yā tu sā chāyaiva śarīra-gā ।।

bhaved yasya praticchāyā chinnā bhinnādhikākulā ।
vi-śirā dvi-śirā jihmā vikṛtā yadi vānya-thā ।।

taṃ samāptāyuṣaṃ vidyān na cel lakṣya-nimitta-jā ।
praticchāyā-mayī yasya na cākṣṇīkṣyeta kanyakā ।।

khādīnāṃ pañca pañcānāṃ chāyā vividha-lakṣaṇāḥ ।
nābhasī nir-malā-nīlā sa-snehā sa-prabheva ca ।।

vātād rajo-'ruṇā śyāvā bhasma-rūkṣā hata-prabhā ।
viśuddha-raktā tv āgneyī dīptābhā darśana-priyā ।।

śuddha-vaiḍūrya-vi-malā su-snigdhā toya-jā sukhā ।
sthirā snigdhā ghanā śuddhā śyāmā śvetā ca pārthivī ।।

u-snigdhā toya-jā hi sā
vāyavī roga-maraṇa-kleśāyānyāḥ sukhodayāḥ ।
prabhoktā taijasī sarvā sā tu sapta-vidhā smṛtā ।।

āyavyā roga-maraṇa-
raktā pītā sitā śyāvā haritā pāṇḍurāsitā ।
tāsāṃ yāḥ syur vikāsinyaḥ snigdhāś ca vi-malāś ca yāḥ ।।

aktā pītā sitā śyāmā
tāḥ śubhā malinā rūkṣāḥ saṃkṣiptāś cā-śubhodayāḥ ।
varṇam ākrāmati cchāyā prabhā varṇa-prakāśinī ।।

aṃkṣiptāś cā-sukhodayāḥ rabhā varṇa-vikāśinī
āsanne lakṣyate chāyā vikṛṣṭe bhā prakāśate ।
nā-cchāyo nā-prabhaḥ kaś-cid viśeṣāś cihnayanti tu ।।

nṛṇāṃ śubhā-śubhotpattiṃ kāle chāyā-samāśrayāḥ ।
nikaṣann iva yaḥ pādau cyutāṃsaḥ parisarpati ।।

āle chāyā-samāśritāḥ
hīyate balataḥ śaśvad yo annam aśnan hitaṃ bahu ।
yo alpāśī bahu-viṇ-mūtro bahv-āśī cālpa-mūtra-viṭ ।।

ahv-āśī vālpa-mūtra-viṭ
yo vālpāśī kaphenārto dīrghaṃ śvasiti ceṣṭate ।
dīrgham ucchvasya yo hrasvaṃ niḥśvasya paritāmyati ।।

hrasvaṃ ca yaḥ praśvasiti vyāviddhaṃ spandate bhṛśam ।
śiro vikṣipate kṛcchrād yo añcayitvā prapāṇikau ।।

yo lalāṭāt sruta-svedaḥ ślatha-saṃdhāna-bandhanaḥ ।
utthāpyamānaḥ saṃmuhyed yo balī dur-balo api vā ।।

uttāna eva svapiti yaḥ pādau vikaroti ca ।
śayanāsana-kuḍyāder yo a-sad eva jighṛkṣati ।।

śayanāsana-kuḍyādau aḥ sadaiva jighṛkṣati
a-hāsya-hāsī saṃmuhyan yo leḍhi daśana-cchadau ।
uttarauṣṭhaṃ parilihan phūt-kārāṃś ca karoti yaḥ ।।

otkārāṃś ca karoti yaḥ
yam abhidravati cchāyā kṛṣṇā pītāruṇāpi vā ।
bhiṣag-bheṣaja-pānānna-guru-mitra-dviṣaś ca ye ।।

ṛṣṇā pītāruṇāpi ca
vaśa-gāḥ sarva evaite vijñeyāḥ sama-vartinaḥ ।
grīvā-lalāṭa-hṛdayaṃ yasya svidyati śītalam ।।

uṣṇo aparaḥ pradeśaś ca śaraṇaṃ tasya devatāḥ ।
yo aṇu-jyotir anekāgro duś-chāyo dur-manāḥ sadā ।।

pūrva-rūpāṇi sarvāṇi jvarādiṣv ati-mātrayā ।
yaṃ viśanti viśaty enaṃ mṛtyur jvara-puraḥ-saraḥ ।।

baliṃ bali-bhṛto yasya praṇītaṃ nopabhuñjate ।
nir-nimittaṃ ca yo medhāṃ śobhām upacayaṃ śriyam ।।

aliṃ bali-bhujo yasya
prāpnoty ato vā vibhraṃśaṃ sa prāpnoti yama-kṣayam ।
guṇa-doṣa-mayī yasya svasthasya vyādhitasya vā ।।

uṇā-guṇa-mayī yasya
yāty anya-thā-tvaṃ prakṛtiḥ ṣaṇ māsān na sa jīvati ।
bhaktiḥ śīlaṃ smṛtis tyāgo buddhir balam a-hetukam ।।

ṣaḍ etāni nivartante ṣaḍbhir māsair mariṣyataḥ ।
matta-vad-gati-vāk-kampa-mohā māsān mariṣyataḥ ।।

naśyaty a-jānan ṣaḍ-ahāt keśa-luñcana-vedanām ।
na yāti yasya cāhāraḥ kaṇṭhaṃ kaṇṭhāmayād ṛte ।।

preṣyāḥ pratīpa-tāṃ yānti pretākṛtir udīryate ।
yasya nidrā bhaven nityā naiva vā na sa jīvati ।।

asya nidrā bhaven nityaṃ
vaktram āpūryate aśrūṇāṃ svidyataś caraṇau bhṛśam ।
cakṣuś cākula-tāṃ yāti yama-rājyaṃ gamiṣyataḥ ।।

ama-rāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyataḥ
yaiḥ purā ramate bhāvair a-ratis tair na jīvati ।
sahasā jāyate yasya vikāraḥ sarva-lakṣaṇaḥ ।।

nivartate vā sahasā sahasā sa vinaśyati ।
jvaro nihanti bala-vān gambhīro dairgharātrikaḥ ।।

sa-pralāpa-bhrama-śvāsaḥ kṣīṇaṃ śūnaṃ hatānalam ।
a-kṣāmaṃ sakta-vacanaṃ raktākṣaṃ hṛdi śūlinam ।।

sa-śuṣka-kāsaḥ pūrvāhṇe yo aparāhṇe api vā bhavet ।
bala-māṃsa-vihīnasya śleṣma-kāsa-samanvitaḥ ।।

aṃśuṣka-kāsaḥ pūrvāhṇe
rakta-pittaṃ bhṛśaṃ raktaṃ kṛṣṇam indra-dhanuṣ-prabham ।
tāmra-hāridra-haritaṃ rūpaṃ raktaṃ pradarśayet ।।

roma-kūpa-pravisṛtaṃ kaṇṭhāsya-hṛdaye sajat ।
vāsaso a-rañjanaṃ pūti vega-vac cāti bhūri ca ।।

āsaso rañjanaṃ pūti
vṛddhaṃ pāṇḍu-jvara-cchardi-kāsa-śophātisāriṇam ।
kāsa-śvāsau jvara-cchardi-tṛṣṇātīsāra-śophinam ।।

yakṣmā pārśva-rujānāha-rakta-cchardy-aṃsa-tāpinam ।
chardir vega-vatī mūtra-śakṛd-gandhiḥ sa-candrikā ।।

-rakta-cchardy-aṅga-tāpinam
sāsra-viṭ-pūya-ruk-kāsa-śvāsa-vaty anuṣaṅgiṇī ।
tṛṣṇānya-roga-kṣapitaṃ bahir-jihvaṃ vi-cetanam ।।

ahir-jihvam a-cetanam ahir-jihvaṃ vi-cetasam
madātyayo ati-śītārtaṃ kṣīṇaṃ taila-prabhānanam ।
arśāṃsi pāṇi-pan-nābhi-guda-muṣkāsya-śophinam ।।

-guda-muṣkādi-śophinam
hṛt-pārśvāṅga-rujā-chardi-pāyu-pāka-jvarāturam ।
atīsāro yakṛt-piṇḍa-māṃsa-dhāvana-mecakaiḥ ।।

tulyas taila-ghṛta-kṣīra-dadhi-majja-vasāsavaiḥ ।
mastuluṅga-maṣī-pūya-vesavārāmbu-mākṣikaiḥ ।।

ati-raktāsita-snigdha-pūty-accha-ghana-vedanaḥ ।
karburaḥ prasravan dhātūn niṣ-purīṣo atha-vāti-viṭ ।।

tantu-mān makṣikākrānto rājī-māṃś candrakair yutaḥ ।
śīrṇa-pāyu-valiṃ mukta-nālaṃ parvāsthi-śūlinam ।।

-tālaṃ parvāsthi-śūlinam -tāḍaṃ parvāsthi-śūlinam
srasta-pāyuṃ bala-kṣīṇam annam evopaveśayan ।
sa-tṛṭ-śvāsa-jvara-cchardi-dāhānāha-pravāhikaḥ ।।

nnam evopaveśayet
aśmarī śūna-vṛṣaṇaṃ baddha-mūtraṃ rujārditam ।
mehas tṛḍ-dāha-piṭikā-māṃsa-kothātisāriṇam ।।

piṭikā marma-hṛt-pṛṣṭha-stanāṃsa-guda-mūrdha-gāḥ ।
parva-pāda-kara-sthā vā mandotsāhaṃ pramehiṇam ।।

-stanāṃsa-guda-mūrdha-jāḥ arva-pāda-kara-sthāś ca
sarvaṃ ca māṃsa-saṃkotha-dāha-tṛṣṇā-mada-jvaraiḥ ।
visarpa-marma-saṃrodha-hidhmā-śvāsa-bhrama-klamaiḥ ।।

arvaṃ ca māṃsa-saṃkoca-
gulmaḥ pṛthu-parīṇāho ghanaḥ kūrma ivonnataḥ ।
sirā-naddho jvara-cchardi-hidhmādhmāna-rujānvitaḥ ।।

kāsa-pīnasa-hṛl-lāsa-śvāsātīsāra-śopha-vān ।
viṇ-mūtra-saṃgraha-śvāsa-śopha-hidhmā-jvara-bhramaiḥ ।।

mūrchā-chardy-atisāraiś ca jaṭharaṃ hanti dur-balam ।
śūnākṣaṃ kuṭilopastham upaklinna-tanu-tvacam ।।

virecana-hṛtānāham ānahyantaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।
pāṇḍu-rogaḥ śvayathu-mān pītākṣi-nakha-darśanam ।।

irecana-hatānāham
tandrā-dāhā-ruci-cchardi-mūrchādhmānātisāra-vān ।
anekopadrava-yutaḥ pādābhyāṃ prasṛto naram ।।

nārīṃ śopho mukhād dhanti kukṣi-guhyād ubhāv api ।
rājī-citaḥ sravaṃś chardi-jvara-śvāsātisāriṇam ।।

jvarātīsārau śophānte śvayathur vā tayoḥ kṣaye ।
dur-balasya viśeṣeṇa jāyante antāya dehinaḥ ।।

śvayathur yasya pāda-sthaḥ parisraste ca piṇḍike ।
sīdataḥ sakthinī caiva taṃ bhiṣak parivarjayet ।।

ānanaṃ hasta-pādaṃ ca viśeṣād yasya śuṣyataḥ ।
śūyete vā vinā dehāt sa māsād yāti pañca-tām ।।

iśeṣād yasya śuṣyati
visarpaḥ kāsa-vaivarṇya-jvara-mūrchāṅga-bhaṅga-vān ।
bhramāsya-śopha-hṛl-lāsa-deha-sādātisāra-vān ।।

hramāsya-śoṣa-hṛl-lāsa-
kuṣṭhaṃ viśīryamāṇāṅgaṃ rakta-netraṃ hata-svaram ।
mandāgniṃ jantubhir juṣṭaṃ hanti tṛṣṇātisāriṇam ।।

vāyuḥ supta-tvacaṃ bhugnaṃ kampa-śopha-rujāturam ।
vātāsraṃ moha-mūrchāya-madā-svapna-jvarānvitam ।।

āyuḥ supta-tvacaṃ bhagnaṃ
śiro-grahā-ruci-śvāsa-saṃkoca-sphoṭa-kotha-vat ।
śiro-rogā-ruci-śvāsa-moha-viḍ-bheda-tṛḍ-bhramaiḥ ।।

ghnanti sarvāmayāḥ kṣīṇa-svara-dhātu-balānalam ।
vāta-vyādhir apasmārī kuṣṭhī rakty udarī kṣayī ।।

gulmī mehī ca tān kṣīṇān vikāre alpe api varjayet ।
bala-māṃsa-kṣayas tīvro roga-vṛddhir a-rocakaḥ ।।

yasyāturasya lakṣyante trīn pakṣān na sa jīvati ।
vātāṣṭhīlāti-saṃvṛddhā tiṣṭhanti dāruṇā hṛdi ।।

tṛṣṇayānuparītasya sadyo muṣṇāti jīvitam ।
śaithilyaṃ piṇḍike vāyur nītvā nāsāṃ ca jihma-tām ।।

ṛṣṇayā tu parītasya
kṣīṇasyāyamya manye vā sadyo muṣṇāti jīvitam ।
nābhi-gudāntaraṃ gatvā vaṅkṣaṇau vā samāśrayan ।।

ṣīṇasyāyasya manye vā
gṛhītvā pāyu-hṛdaye kṣīṇa-dehasya vā balī ।
malān vasti-śiro nābhiṃ vibadhya janayan rujam ।।

kurvan vaṅkṣaṇayoḥ śūlaṃ tṛṣṇāṃ bhinna-purīṣa-tām ।
śvāsaṃ vā janayan vāyur gṛhītvā guda-vaṅkṣaṇam ।।

ṛhītvā guda-vaṅkṣaṇau
vitatya parśukāgrāṇi gṛhītvoraś ca mārutaḥ ।
stimitasyātatākṣasya sadyo muṣṇāti jīvitam ।।

itatya pārśvakāgrāṇi
sahasā jvara-saṃtāpas tṛṣṇā mūrchā bala-kṣayaḥ ।
viśleṣaṇaṃ ca saṃdhīnāṃ mumūrṣor upajāyate ।।

go-sarge vadanād yasya svedaḥ pracyavate bhṛśam ।
lepa-jvaropataptasya dur-labhaṃ tasya jīvitam ।।

pravāla-guṭikābhāsā yasya gātre masūrikāḥ ।
utpadyāśu vinaśyanti na cirāt sa vinaśyati ।।

masūra-vidala-prakhyās tathā vidruma-saṃnibhāḥ ।
antar-vaktrāḥ kiṇābhāś ca visphoṭā deha-nāśanāḥ ।।

kāmalākṣṇor mukhaṃ pūrṇaṃ śaṅkhayor mukta-māṃsa-tā ।
saṃtrāsaś coṣṇa-tāṅge ca yasya taṃ parivarjayet ।।

a-kasmād anudhāvac ca vighṛṣṭaṃ tvak-samāśrayam ।
yo vāta-jo na śūlāya syān na dāhāya pitta-jaḥ ।।

candanośīra-madirā-kuṇapa-dhvāṅkṣa-gandhayaḥ ।
śaivāla-kukkuṭa-śikhā-kuṅkumāla-maṣī-prabhāḥ ।।

-naktamāla-maṣī-prabhāḥ -kunda-śāli-maya-prabhāḥ antar-dāhā nir-ūṣmaṇaḥ prāṇa-nāśa-karā vraṇāḥ ।।

kapha-jo na ca pūyāya marma-jaś ca ruje na yaḥ ।
a-cūrṇaś cūrṇa-kīrṇābho yatrākasmāc ca dṛśyate ।।

rūpaṃ śakti-dhvajādīnāṃ sarvāṃs tān varjayed vraṇān ।
viṇ-mūtra-māruta-vahaṃ kṛmiṇaṃ ca bhagandaram ।।

ghaṭṭayañ jānunā jānu pādāv udyamya pātayan ।
yo apāsyati muhur vaktram āturo na sa jīvati ।।

dantaiś chindan nakhāgrāṇi taiś ca keśāṃs tṛṇāni ca ।
bhūmiṃ kāṣṭhena vilikhan loṣṭaṃ loṣṭena tāḍayan ।।

aiś ca keśāṃs tṛṇāni vā
hṛṣṭa-romā sāndra-mūtraḥ śuṣka-kāsī jvarī ca yaḥ ।
muhur hasan muhuḥ kṣveḍan śayyāṃ pādena hanti yaḥ ।।

śayyāṃ pādena hanti ca
muhuś chidrāṇi vimṛśann āturo na sa jīvati ।
mṛtyave sahasārtasya tilaka-vyaṅga-viplavaḥ ।।

mukhe danta-nakhe puṣpaṃ jaṭhare vividhāḥ sirāḥ ।
ūrdhva-śvāsaṃ gatoṣmāṇaṃ śūlopahata-vaṅkṣaṇam ।।

śarma cān-adhigacchantaṃ buddhi-mān parivarjayet ।
vikārā yasya vardhante prakṛtiḥ parihīyate ।।

śarma vān-adhigacchantaṃ
sahasā sahasā tasya mṛtyur harati jīvitam ।
yam uddiśyāturaṃ vaidyaḥ saṃpādayitum auṣadham ।।

yatamāno na śaknoti dur-labhaṃ tasya jīvitam ।
vijñātaṃ bahu-śaḥ siddhaṃ vidhi-vac cāvacāritam ।।

na sidhyaty auṣadhaṃ yasya nāsti tasya cikitsitam ।
bhaved yasyauṣadhe anne vā kalpyamāne viparyayaḥ ।।

a-kasmād varṇa-gandhādeḥ svastho api na sa jīvati ।
nivāte sendhanaṃ yasya jyotiś cāpy upaśāmyati ।।

āturasya gṛhe yasya bhidyante vā patanti vā ।
ati-mātram amatrāṇi dur-labhaṃ tasya jīvitam ।।

yaṃ naraṃ sahasā rogo dur-balaṃ parimuñcati ।
saṃśaya-prāptam ātreyo jīvitaṃ tasya manyate ।।

aṃśayaṃ prāptam ātreyo
kathayen na ca pṛṣṭo api duḥ-śravaṃ maraṇaṃ bhiṣak ।
gatāsor bandhu-mitrāṇāṃ na cecchet taṃ cikitsitum ।।

athayen naiva pṛṣṭo api
yama-dūta-piśācādyair yat parāsur upāsyate ।
ghnadbhir auṣadha-vīryāṇi tasmāt taṃ parivarjayet ।।

āyur-veda-phalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ yad āyur-jñe pratiṣṭhitam ।
riṣṭa-jñānādṛtas tasmāt sarva-daiva bhaved bhiṣak ।।

maraṇaṃ prāṇināṃ dṛṣṭam āyuḥ-puṇyobhaya-kṣayāt ।
tayor apy a-kṣayād dṛṣṭaṃ viṣamā-parihāriṇām ।।

”ārīrasthāna
pāṣaṇḍāśrama-varṇānāṃ sa-varṇāḥ karma-siddhaye ।
ta eva viparītāḥ syur dūtāḥ karma-vipattaye ।।

dīnaṃ bhītaṃ drutaṃ trastaṃ rūkṣā-maṅgala-vādinam ।
śastriṇaṃ daṇḍinaṃ ṣaṇḍhaṃ muṇḍa-śmaśru-jaṭā-dharam ।।

śastriṇaṃ daṇḍinaṃ khaṇḍaṃ uṇḍa-śmaśruṃ jaṭā-dharam 
uṇḍaṃ śmaśru-jaṭā-dharam
a-maṅgalāhvayaṃ krūra-karmāṇaṃ malinaṃ striyam ।
anekaṃ vyādhitaṃ vyaṅgaṃ rakta-mālyānulepanam ।।

taila-paṅkāṅkitaṃ jīrṇa-vi-varṇārdraika-vāsasam ।
kharoṣṭra-mahiṣārūḍhaṃ kāṣṭha-loṣṭādi-mardinam ।।

āṣṭha-lohādi-mardinam
nānugacched bhiṣag dūtam āhvayantaṃ ca dūrataḥ ।
a-śasta-cintā-vacane nagne chindati bhindati ।।

juhvāne pāvakaṃ piṇḍān pitṛbhyo nirvapaty api ।
supte mukta-kace abhyakte rudaty a-prayate tathā ।।

udaty a-prayate atha-vā
vaidye dūtā manuṣyāṇām āgacchanti mumūrṣatām ।
vikāra-sāmānya-guṇe deśe kāle atha-vā bhiṣak ।।

dūtam abhyāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā nāturaṃ tam upācaret ।
spṛśanto nābhi-nāsāsya-keśa-roma-nakha-dvi-jān ।।

pṛśanto nābhi-nāsākṣi-
guhya-pṛṣṭha-stana-grīvā-jaṭharānāmikāṅgulīḥ ।
kārpāsa-busa-sīsāsthi-kapāla-musalopalam ।।

-jaṭharānāmikāṅguli
mārjanī-śūrpa-cailānta-bhasmāṅgāra-daśā-tuṣān ।
rajjūpānat-tulā-pāśam anyad vā bhagna-vicyutam ।।

nyad vā bhagna-vidyutam
tat-pūrva-darśane dūtā vyāharanti mariṣyatām ।
tathārdha-rātre madhyāhne saṃdhyayoḥ parva-vāsare ।।

ṣaṣṭhī-caturthī-navamī-rāhu-ketūdayādiṣu ।
bharaṇī-kṛttikāśleṣā-pūrvārdrā-paitrya-nairṛte ।।

yasmiṃś ca dūte bruvati vākyam ātura-saṃśrayam ।
paśyen nimittam a-śubhaṃ taṃ ca nānuvrajed bhiṣak ।।

tad yathā vikalaḥ pretaḥ pretālaṅkāra eva vā ।
chinnaṃ dagdhaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ vā tad-vādīni vacāṃsi vā ।।

retālaṅkāra eva ca
raso vā kaṭukas tīvro gandho vā kauṇapo mahān ।
sparśo vā vipulaḥ krūro yad vānyad api tādṛśam ।।

parśo vā vipula-krūro
tat sarvam abhito vākyaṃ vākya-kāle atha-vā punaḥ ।
dūtam abhyāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā nāturaṃ tam upācaret ।।

hāhā-kranditam utkruṣṭam ākruṣṭaṃ skhalanaṃ kṣutam ।
vastrātapa-tra-pāda-tra-vyasanaṃ vyasanīkṣaṇam ।।

caitya-dhvajānāṃ pātrāṇāṃ pūrṇānāṃ ca nimajjanam ।
hatān-iṣṭa-pravādāś ca dūṣaṇaṃ bhasma-pāṃsubhiḥ ।।

pathaś chedo ahi-mārjāra-godhā-saraṭa-vānaraiḥ ।
dīptāṃ prati diśaṃ vācaḥ krūrāṇāṃ mṛga-pakṣiṇām ।।

kṛṣṇa-dhānya-guḍodaśvil-lavaṇāsava-carmaṇām ।
sarṣapāṇāṃ vasā-taila-tṛṇa-paṅkendhanasya ca ।।

klība-krūra-śva-pākānāṃ jāla-vāgurayor api ।
charditasya purīṣasya pūti-dur-darśanasya ca ।।

niḥ-sārasya vyavāyasya kārpāsāder arer api ।
śayanāsana-yānānām uttānānāṃ tu darśanam ।।

ttānānāṃ ca darśanam
nyubjānām itareṣāṃ ca pātrādīnām a-śobhanam ।
puṃ-saṃjñāḥ pakṣiṇo vāmāḥ strī-saṃjñā dakṣiṇāḥ śubhāḥ ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ khaga-mṛgā yānto naivaṃ śva-jambukāḥ ।
a-yugmāś ca mṛgāḥ śastāḥ śastā nityaṃ ca darśane ।।

cāṣa-bhāsa-bharadvāja-nakula-cchāga-barhiṇaḥ ।
a-śubhaṃ sarva-tholūka-biḍāla-saraṭekṣaṇam ।।

praśastāḥ kīrtane kola-godhāhi-śaśa-jāhakāḥ ।
na darśane na virute vānararkṣāv ato anya-thā ।।

dhanur aindraṃ ca lālāṭam a-śubhaṃ śubham anyataḥ ।
agni-pūrṇāni pātrāṇi bhinnāni vi-śikhāni ca ।।

dadhy-a-kṣatādi nirgacchad vakṣyamāṇaṃ ca maṅgalam ।
vaidyo mariṣyatāṃ veśma praviśann eva paśyati ।।

dūtādy a-sādhu dṛṣṭvaivaṃ tyajed ārtam ato anya-thā ।
karuṇā-śuddha-saṃtāno yatnatas tam upācaret ।।

atnataḥ samupācaret
dadhy-a-kṣatekṣu-niṣpāva-priyaṅgu-madhu-sarpiṣām ।
yāvakāñjana-bhṛṅgāra-ghaṇṭā-dīpa-saro-ruhām ।।

dūrvārdra-matsya-māṃsānāṃ lājānāṃ phala-bhakṣayoḥ ।
ratnebha-pūrṇa-kumbhānāṃ kanyāyāḥ syandanasya ca ।।

narasya vardhamānasya devatānāṃ nṛpasya ca ।
śuklānāṃ su-mano-vāla-cāmarāmbara-vājinām ।।

śaṅkha-sādhu-dvi-joṣṇīṣa-toraṇa-svastikasya ca ।
bhūmeḥ samuddhatāyāś ca vahneḥ prajvalitasya ca ।।

mano-jñasyānna-pānasya pūrṇasya śakaṭasya ca ।
nṛbhir dhenvāḥ sa-vatsāyā vaḍabāyāḥ striyā api ।।

jīvañjīvaka-sāraṅga-sārasa-priyavādinām ।
haṃsānāṃ śatapattrāṇāṃ baddhasyaika-paśos tathā ।।

rucakādarśa-siddhārtha-rocanānāṃ ca darśanam ।
gandhaḥ su-surabhir varṇaḥ su-śuklo madhuro rasaḥ ।।

go-pater anukūlasya svanas tad-vad gavām api ।
mṛga-pakṣi-narāṇāṃ ca śobhināṃ śobhanā giraḥ ।।

o-pater anulomasya
chattra-dhvaja-patākānām utkṣepaṇam abhiṣṭutiḥ ।
bherī-mṛdaṅga-śaṅkhānāṃ śabdāḥ puṇyāha-niḥsvanāḥ ।।

vedādhyayana-śabdāś ca sukho vāyuḥ pradakṣiṇaḥ ।
pathi veśma-praveśe ca vidyād ārogya-lakṣaṇam ।।

ity uktaṃ dūta-śakunaṃ svapnān ūrdhvaṃ pracakṣate ।
svapne madyaṃ saha pretair yaḥ piban kṛṣyate śunā ।।

vapnān ūrdhvaṃ pracakṣyate vapnān ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyate
sa martyo mṛtyunā śīghraṃ jvara-rūpeṇa nīyate ।
rakta-mālya-vapur-vastro yo hasan hriyate striyā ।।

a martyo mṛtyunā tūrṇaṃ
so asra-pittena mahiṣa-śva-varāhoṣṭra-gardabhaiḥ ।
yaḥ prayāti diśaṃ yāmyāṃ maraṇaṃ tasya yakṣmaṇā ।।

latā kaṇṭakinī vaṃśas tālo vā hṛdi jāyate ।
yasya tasyāśu gulmena yasya vahnim an-arciṣam ।।

juhvato ghṛta-siktasya nagnasyorasi jāyate ।
padmaṃ sa naśyet kuṣṭhena caṇḍālaiḥ saha yaḥ pibet ।।

snehaṃ bahu-vidhaṃ svapne sa prameheṇa naśyati ।
unmādena jale majjed yo nṛtyan rākṣasaiḥ saha ।।

apasmāreṇa yo martyo nṛtyan pretena nīyate ।
yānaṃ kharoṣṭra-mārjāra-kapi-śārdūla-śūkaraiḥ ।।

yasya pretaiḥ śṛgālair vā sa mṛtyor vartate mukhe ।
apūpa-śaṣkulīr jagdhvā vibuddhas tad-vidhaṃ vaman ।।

na jīvaty akṣi-rogāya sūryendu-grahaṇekṣaṇam ।
sūryā-candramasoḥ pāta-darśanaṃ dṛg-vināśanam ।।

mūrdhni vaṃśa-latādīnāṃ saṃbhavo vayasāṃ tathā ।
nilayo muṇḍa-tā kāka-gṛdhrādyaiḥ parivāraṇam ।।

tathā preta-piśāca-strī-draviḍāndhra-gavāśanaiḥ ।
saṅgo vetra-latā-vaṃśa-tṛṇa-kaṇṭaka-saṃkaṭe ।।

śvabhra-śmaśāna-śayanaṃ patanaṃ pāṃsu-bhasmanoḥ ।
majjanaṃ jala-paṅkādau śīghreṇa srotasā hṛtiḥ ।।

nṛtya-vāditra-gītāni rakta-srag-vastra-dhāraṇam ।
vayo-'ṅga-vṛddhir abhyaṅgo vivāhaḥ śmaśru-karma ca ।।

pakvānna-sneha-madyāśaḥ pracchardana-virecane ।
hiraṇya-lohayor lābhaḥ kalir bandha-parājayau ।।

racchardana-virecanam
upānad-yuga-nāśaś ca prapātaḥ pāda-carmaṇoḥ ।
harṣo bhṛśaṃ prakupitaiḥ pitṛbhiś cāvabhartsanam ।।

pradīpa-graha-nakṣatra-danta-daivata-cakṣuṣām ।
patanaṃ vā vināśo vā bhedanaṃ parvatasya ca ।।

hedanaṃ parvatasya vā
kānane rakta-kusume pāpa-karma-niveśane ।
citāndha-kāra-saṃbādhe jananyāṃ ca praveśanam ।।

c cintāndha-kāra-saṃbādhe
pātaḥ prāsāda-śailāder matsyena grasanaṃ tathā ।
kāṣāyiṇām a-saumyānāṃ nagnānāṃ daṇḍa-dhāriṇām ।।

raktākṣāṇāṃ ca kṛṣṇānāṃ darśanaṃ jātu neṣyate ।
kṛṣṇā pāpānanācārā dīrgha-keśa-nakha-stanī ।।

vi-rāga-mālya-vasanā svapne kāla-niśā matā ।
mano-vahānāṃ pūrṇa-tvāt srotasāṃ prabalair malaiḥ ।।

dṛśyante dāruṇāḥ svapnā rogī yair yāti pañca-tām ।
a-rogaḥ saṃśayaṃ prāpya kaś-cid eva vimucyate ।।

dṛṣṭaḥ śruto anubhūtaś ca prārthitaḥ kalpitas tathā ।
bhāviko doṣa-jaś ceti svapnaḥ sapta-vidho mataḥ ।।

vapnaḥ sapta-vidhaḥ smṛtaḥ
teṣv ādyā niṣ-phalāḥ pañca yathā-sva-prakṛtir divā ।
vismṛto dīrgha-hrasvo ati pūrva-rātre cirāt phalam ।।

athā-svaṃ prakṛtir divā ismṛto dīrgha-hrasvo api 
vismṛto dīrgha-hrasvo vā
dṛṣṭaḥ karoti tucchaṃ ca go-sarge tad-ahar mahat ।
nidrayā vān-upahataḥ pratīpair vacanais tathā ।।

ṛṣṭaḥ karoti tucchaṃ vā idrayā cān-upahataḥ
yāti pāpo alpa-phala-tāṃ dāna-homa-japādibhiḥ ।
a-kalyāṇam api svapnaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatraiva yaḥ punaḥ ।।

āti pāpo apy a-phala-tāṃ
paśyet saumyaṃ śubhaṃ tasya śubham eva phalaṃ bhavet ।
devān dvi-jān go-vṛṣabhān jīvataḥ suhṛdo nṛpān ।।

sādhūn yaśasvino vahnim iddhaṃ svacchān jalāśayān ।
kanyāḥ kumārakān gaurān śukla-vastrān su-tejasaḥ ।।

anyāṃ kumārakān gaurān
narāśanaṃ dīpta-tanuṃ samantād rudhirokṣitam ।
yaḥ paśyel labhate yo vā chattrādarśa-viṣāmiṣam ।।

arāśanaṃ dīpta-tanuḥ amantād rudhirokṣitaḥ
śuklāḥ su-manaso vastram a-medhyālepanaṃ phalam ।
śaila-prāsāda-sa-phala-vṛkṣa-siṃha-nara-dvi-pān ।।

ārohed go-'śva-yānaṃ ca taren nada-hradoda-dhīn ।
pūrvottareṇa gamanam a-gamyāgamanaṃ mṛtam ।।

aren nada-mahoda-dhīn
saṃbādhān niḥsṛtir devaiḥ pitṛbhiś cābhinandanam ।
rodanaṃ patitotthānaṃ dviṣatāṃ cāvamardanam ।।

aṃkaṭān niḥsṛtir devaiḥ viṣatāṃ cāpamardanam
yasya syād āyur ārogyaṃ vittaṃ bahu ca so aśnute ।
maṅgalācāra-saṃpannaḥ parivāras tathāturaḥ ।।

ittaṃ sa bahu-śo aśnute
śrad-dadhāno anukūlaś ca prabhūta-dravya-saṃgrahaḥ ।
sat-tva-lakṣaṇa-saṃyogo bhaktir vaidya-dvi-jātiṣu ।।

cikitsāyām a-nirvedas tad ārogyasya lakṣaṇam ।
ity atra janma-maraṇaṃ yataḥ samyag udāhṛtam ।।
śarīrasya tataḥ sthānaṃ śārīram idam ucyate ।।
nidānasthāna
rogaḥ pāpmā jvaro vyādhir vikāro duḥkham āmayaḥ ।
yakṣmātaṅka-gadābādhāḥ śabdāḥ paryāya-vācinaḥ ।।

nidānaṃ pūrva-rūpāṇi rūpāṇy upaśayas tathā ।
saṃprāptiś ceti vijñānaṃ rogāṇāṃ pañca-dhā smṛtam ।।

nimitta-hetv-āyatana-pratyayotthāna-kāraṇaiḥ ।
nidānam āhuḥ paryāyaiḥ prāg-rūpaṃ yena lakṣyate ।।

utpitsur āmayo doṣa-viśeṣeṇān-adhiṣṭhitaḥ ।
liṅgam a-vyaktam alpa-tvād vyādhīnāṃ tad yathā-yatham ।।

tad eva vyakta-tāṃ yātaṃ rūpam ity abhidhīyate ।
saṃsthānaṃ vyañjanaṃ liṅgaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ cihnam ākṛtiḥ ।।

hetu-vyādhi-viparyasta-viparyastārtha-kāriṇām ।
auṣadhānna-vihārāṇām upayogaṃ sukhāvaham ।।

vidyād upaśayaṃ vyādheḥ sa hi sātmyam iti smṛtaḥ ।
viparīto an-upaśayo vyādhy-a-sātmyābhisaṃjñitaḥ ।।

yathā-duṣṭena doṣeṇa yathā cānuvisarpatā ।
nirvṛttir āmayasyāsau saṃprāptir jātir āgatiḥ ।।

saṃkhyā-vikalpa-prādhānya-bala-kāla-viśeṣataḥ ।
sā bhidyate yathātraiva vakṣyante aṣṭau jvarā iti ।।

doṣāṇāṃ samavetānāṃ vikalpo aṃśāṃśa-kalpanā ।
svātantrya-pāratantryābhyāṃ vyādheḥ prādhānyam ādiśet ।।

hetv-ādi-kārtsnyāvayavair balā-bala-viśeṣaṇam ।
naktan-dinartu-bhuktāṃśair vyādhi-kālo yathā-malam ।।

iti prokto nidānārthas taṃ vyāsenopadekṣyati ।
sarveṣām eva rogāṇāṃ nidānaṃ kupitā malāḥ ।।

ti prokto nidānārthaḥ aṃ vyāsenopadekṣyate aṃ vyāsenopadiśyate a vyāsenopadekṣyati a vyāsenopadekṣyate a 
vyāsenopadiśyate
tat-prakopasya tu proktaṃ vividhā-hita-sevanam ।
a-hitaṃ tri-vidho yogas trayāṇāṃ prāg udāhṛtaḥ ।।

-hitas tri-vidho yogas
tiktoṣaṇa-kaṣāyālpa-rūkṣa-pramita-bhojanaiḥ ।
dhāraṇodīraṇa-niśā-jāgarāty-ucca-bhāṣaṇaiḥ ।।

kriyāti-yoga-bhī-śoka-cintā-vyāyāma-maithunaiḥ ।
grīṣmāho-rātri-bhuktānte prakupyati samīraṇaḥ ।।

pittaṃ kaṭv-amla-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-paṭu-krodha-vidāhibhiḥ ।
śaran-madhyāhna-rātry-ardha-vidāha-samayeṣu ca ।।

-nidāgha-samayeṣu ca
svādv-amla-lavaṇa-snigdha-gurv-abhiṣyandi-śītalaiḥ ।
āsyā-svapna-sukhā-jīrṇa-divā-svapnāti-bṛṃhaṇaiḥ ।।

ti-svapna-sukhā-jīrṇa-
pracchardanādya-yogena bhukta-mātra-vasantayoḥ ।
pūrvāhṇe pūrva-rātre ca śleṣmā dvandvaṃ tu saṃkarāt ।।

miśrī-bhāvāt samastānāṃ saṃnipātas tathā punaḥ ।
saṃkīrṇā-jīrṇa-viṣama-viruddhādhyaśanādibhiḥ ।।

vyāpanna-madya-pānīya-śuṣka-śākāma-mūlakaiḥ ।
piṇyāka-mṛd-yava-surā-pūti-śuṣka-kṛśāmiṣaiḥ ।।

doṣa-traya-karais tais tais tathānna-parivartanāt ।
ṛtor duṣṭāt puro-vātād grahāveśād viṣād garāt ।।

athānna-parivartataḥ athānna-parivṛttitaḥ
duṣṭānnāt parvatāśleṣād grahair janmarkṣa-pīḍanāt ।
mithyā-yogāc ca vividhāt pāpānāṃ ca niṣevaṇāt ।।

uṣṭāmāt parvatāśleṣād
strīṇāṃ prasava-vaiṣamyāt tathā mithyopacārataḥ ।
prati-rogam iti kruddhā rogādhiṣṭhāna-gāminīḥ ।।
rasāyanīḥ prapadyāśu doṣā dehe vikurvate ।।
nidānasthāna
jvaro roga-patiḥ pāpmā mṛtyur ojo-'śano antakaḥ ।
krodho dakṣādhvara-dhvaṃsī rudrordhva-nayanodbhavaḥ ।।

ṛtyus tejo-'śano antakaḥ
janmāntayor moha-mayaḥ saṃtāpātmāpacāra-jaḥ ।
vividhair nāmabhiḥ krūro nānā-yoniṣu vartate ।।

sa jāyate aṣṭa-dhā doṣaiḥ pṛthaṅ miśraiḥ samāgataiḥ ।
āgantuś ca malās tatra svaiḥ svair duṣṭāḥ pradūṣaṇaiḥ ।।

āmāśayaṃ praviśyāmam anugamya pidhāya ca ।
srotāṃsi pakti-sthānāc ca nirasya jvalanaṃ bahiḥ ।।

saha tenābhisarpantas tapantaḥ sakalaṃ vapuḥ ।
kurvanto gātram aty-uṣṇaṃ jvaraṃ nirvartayanti te ।।

urvanto gātram ā-śuṣkaṃ
sroto-vibandhāt prāyeṇa tataḥ svedo na jāyate ।
tasya prāg-rūpam ālasyam a-ratir gātra-gauravam ।।

āsya-vairasyam a-ruci-jṛmbhā sāsrākulākṣi-tā ।
aṅga-mardo a-vipāko alpa-prāṇa-tā bahu-nidra-tā ।।

-jṛmbhā sāsrākulākṣa-tā
roma-harṣo vinamanaṃ piṇḍikodveṣṭanaṃ klamaḥ ।
hitopadeśeṣv a-kṣāntiḥ prītir amla-paṭūṣaṇe ।।

dveṣaḥ svāduṣu bhakṣyeṣu tathā bāleṣu tṛḍ bhṛśam ।
śabdāgni-śīta-vātāmbu-cchāyoṣṇeṣv a-nimittataḥ ।।

icchā dveṣaś ca tad anu jvarasya vyakta-tā bhavet ।
āgamāpagama-kṣobha-mṛdu-tā-vedanoṣmaṇām ।।

vaiṣamyaṃ tatra tatrāṅge tās tāḥ syur vedanāś calāḥ ।
pādayoḥ supta-tā stambhaḥ piṇḍikodveṣṭanaṃ śamaḥ ।।

iṇḍikodveṣṭanaṃ klamaḥ
viśleṣa iva saṃdhīnāṃ sāda ūrvoḥ kaṭī-grahaḥ ।
pṛṣṭhaṃ kṣodam ivāpnoti niṣpīḍyata ivodaram ।।

chidyanta iva cāsthīni pārśva-gāni viśeṣataḥ ।
hṛdayasya grahas todaḥ prājaneneva vakṣasaḥ ।।

skandhayor mathanaṃ bāhvor bhedaḥ pīḍanam aṃsayoḥ ।
a-śaktir bhakṣaṇe hanvor jṛmbhaṇaṃ karṇayoḥ svanaḥ ।।

nistodaḥ śaṅkhayor mūrdhni vedanā vi-rasāsya-tā ।
kaṣāyāsya-tvam atha-vā malānām a-pravartanam ।।

rūkṣāruṇa-tvag-āsyākṣi-nakha-mūtra-purīṣa-tā ।
prasekā-rocakā-śraddhā-vipākā-sveda-jāgarāḥ ।।

kaṇṭhauṣṭha-śoṣas tṛṭ śuṣkau chardi-kāsau viṣādi-tā ।
harṣo romāṅga-danteṣu vepathuḥ kṣavathor grahaḥ ।।

śvayathuḥ kṣavathor grahaḥ
bhramaḥ pralāpo gharmecchā vināmaś cānila-jvare ।
yuga-pad vyāptir aṅgānāṃ pralāpaḥ kaṭu-vaktra-tā ।।

nāsāsya-pākaḥ śītecchā bhramo mūrchā mado a-ratiḥ ।
viṭ-sraṃsaḥ pitta-vamanaṃ rakta-ṣṭhīvanam amlakaḥ ।।

rakta-koṭhodgamaḥ pīta-harita-tvaṃ tvag-ādiṣu ।
svedo niḥśvāsa-vaigandhyam ati-tṛṣṇā ca pitta-je ।।

viśeṣād a-rucir jāḍyaṃ sroto-rodho alpa-vega-tā ।
praseko mukha-mādhuryaṃ hṛl-lepa-śvāsa-pīnasāḥ ।।

hṛl-lāsaś chardanaṃ kāsaḥ stambhaḥ śvaityaṃ tvag-ādiṣu ।
aṅgeṣu śīta-piṭikās tandrodardaḥ kaphodbhave ।।
kāle yathā-svaṃ sarveṣāṃ pravṛttir vṛddhir eva vā ।।nidānoktān-upaśayo viparītopaśāyi-tā ।।yathā-svaṃ liṅga-saṃsarge jvaraḥ saṃsarga-jo api ca ।।
śiro-'rti-mūrchā-vami-dāha-moha-kaṇṭhāsya-śoṣā-rati-parva-bhedāḥ ।
unnidra-tā-tṛḍ-bhrama-roma-harṣā jṛmbhāti-vāk-tvaṃ ca calāt sa-pittāt ।।

tāpa-hāny-a-ruci-parva-śiro-ruk-pīnasa-śvasana-kāsa-vibandhāḥ ।
śīta-jāḍya-timira-bhrama-tandrāḥ śleṣma-vāta-janita-jvara-liṅgam ।।

śīta-stambha-sveda-dāhā-vyavasthā tṛṣṇā-kāsa-śleṣma-pitta-pravṛttiḥ ।
mohas tandrā lipta-tiktāsya-tā ca jñeyaṃ rūpaṃ śleṣma-pitta-jvarasya ।।

ṛṣṇā kāsaḥ śleṣma-pitta-pravṛttiḥ
sarva-jo lakṣaṇaiḥ sarvair dāho atra ca muhur muhuḥ ।
tad-vac chītaṃ mahā-nidrā divā jāgaraṇaṃ niśi ।।

sadā vā naiva vā nidrā mahā-svedo ati naiva vā ।
gīta-nartana-hāsyādi-vikṛtehā-pravartanam ।।

ahān svedo ati naiva vā
sāśruṇī kaluṣe rakte bhugne lulita-pakṣmaṇī ।
akṣiṇī piṇḍikā-pārśva-mūrdha-parvāsthi-rug-bhramaḥ ।।

sa-svanau sa-rujau karṇau kaṇṭhaḥ śūkair ivācitaḥ ।
paridagdhā kharā jihvā guru-srastāṅga-saṃdhi-tā ।।

uruḥ srastāṅga-saṃdhi-tā
rakta-pitta-kapha-ṣṭhīvo lolanaṃ śiraso ati-ruk ।
koṭhānāṃ śyāva-raktānāṃ maṇḍalānāṃ ca darśanam ।।

olanaṃ śiraso ati-tṛṭ
hṛd-vyathā mala-saṃsaṅgaḥ pravṛttir vālpa-śo ati vā ।
snigdhāsya-tā bala-bhraṃśaḥ svara-sādaḥ pralāpi-tā ।।

ṛd-vyathā mala-saṃsargaḥ
doṣa-pākaś cirāt tandrā pratataṃ kaṇṭha-kūjanam ।
saṃnipātam abhinyāsaṃ taṃ brūyāc ca hṛtaujasam ।।

aṃ brūyāc ca hataujasam
vāyunā kapha-ruddhena pittam antaḥ prapīḍitam ।
vyavāyi-tvāc ca sūkṣma-tvād bahir-mārgaṃ pravartate ।।
tena hāridra-netra-tvaṃ saṃnipātodbhave jvare ।।
doṣe vibaddhe naṣṭe agnau sarva-saṃpūrṇa-lakṣaṇaḥ ।
a-sādhyaḥ so anya-thā kṛcchro bhaved vaikalya-do api vā ।।

anyac ca saṃnipātottho yatra pittaṃ pṛthak sthitam ।
tvaci koṣṭhe atha-vā dāhaṃ vidadhāti puro anu vā ।।

nyaś ca saṃnipātottho
tad-vad vāta-kaphau śītaṃ dāhādir dus-taras tayoḥ ।
śītādau tatra pittena kaphe syandita-śoṣite ।।

śīte śānte amlako mūrchā madas tṛṣṇā ca jāyate ।
dāhādau punar ante syus tandrā-ṣṭhīva-vami-klamāḥ ।।

āgantur abhighātābhiṣaṅga-śāpābhicārataḥ ।
catur-dhātra kṣata-ccheda-dāhādyair abhighāta-jaḥ ।।

śramāc ca tasmin pavanaḥ prāyo raktaṃ pradūṣayan ।
sa-vyathā-śopha-vaivarṇyaṃ sa-rujaṃ kurute jvaram ।।

grahāveśauṣadhi-viṣa-krodha-bhī-śoka-kāma-jaḥ ।
abhiṣaṅgād graheṇāsminn a-kasmād dhāsa-rodane ।।

oṣadhi-gandha-je mūrchā śiro-rug vamathuḥ kṣavaḥ ।
viṣān mūrchātisārāsya-śyāva-tā-dāha-hṛd-gadāḥ ।।

śiro-ruk śvayathuḥ kṣavaḥ śiro-rug vepathuḥ kṣavaḥ 
-śyāva-tā-dāha-hṛd-grahāḥ
krodhāt kampaḥ śiro-ruk ca pralāpo bhaya-śoka-je ।
kāmād bhramo a-rucir dāho hrī-nidrā-dhī-dhṛti-kṣayaḥ ।।

hī-nidrā-dhī-dhṛti-kṣayaḥ
grahādau saṃnipātasya bhayādau marutas traye ।
kopaḥ kope api pittasya yau tu śāpābhicāra-jau ।।

opaḥ kope tu pittasya opaḥ krodhe tu pittasya
saṃnipāta-jvarau ghorau tāv a-sahya-tamau matau ।
tatrābhicārikair mantrair hūyamānasya tapyate ।।

āv a-sādhya-tamau matau
pūrvaṃ cetas tato dehas tato visphoṭa-tṛḍ-bhramaiḥ ।
sa-dāha-mūrchair grastasya praty-ahaṃ vardhate jvaraḥ ।।

iti jvaro aṣṭa-dhā dṛṣṭaḥ samāsād vividhas tu saḥ ।
śārīro mānasaḥ saumyas tīkṣṇo antar-bahir-āśrayaḥ ।।

prākṛto vaikṛtaḥ sādhyo a-sādhyaḥ sāmo nir-āmakaḥ ।
pūrvaṃ śarīre śārīre tāpo manasi mānase ।।

pavane yoga-vāhi-tvāc chītaṃ śleṣma-yute bhavet ।
dāhaḥ pitta-yute miśraṃ miśre antaḥ-saṃśraye punaḥ ।।

jvare adhikaṃ vikārāḥ syur antaḥ kṣobho mala-grahaḥ ।
bahir eva bahir-vege tāpo api ca su-sādhya-tā ।।

varṣā-śarad-vasanteṣu vātādyaiḥ prākṛtaḥ kramāt ।
vaikṛto anyaḥ sa duḥ-sādhyaḥ prāyaś ca prākṛto anilāt ।।

varṣāsu māruto duṣṭaḥ pitta-śleṣmānvito jvaram ।
kuryāt pittaṃ ca śaradi tasya cānu-balaṃ kaphaḥ ।।

asya cānu-balaḥ kaphaḥ
tat-prakṛtyā visargāc ca tatra nān-aśanād bhayam ।
kapho vasante tam api vāta-pittaṃ bhaved anu ।।

at-prakṛtyā visargasya
bala-vatsv alpa-doṣeṣu jvaraḥ sādhyo an-upadravaḥ ।
sarva-thā vikṛti-jñāne prāg a-sādhya udāhṛtaḥ ।।

jvaropadrava-tīkṣṇa-tvam a-glānir bahu-mūtra-tā ।
na pravṛttir na viḍ jīrṇā na kṣut sāma-jvarākṛtiḥ ।।

jvara-vego adhikaṃ tṛṣṇā pralāpaḥ śvasanaṃ bhramaḥ ।
mala-pravṛttir utkleśaḥ pacyamānasya lakṣaṇam ।।

vara-vego adhikas tṛṣṇā
jīrṇa-tāma-viparyāsāt sapta-rātraṃ ca laṅghanāt ।
jvaraḥ pañca-vidhaḥ prokto mala-kāla-balā-balāt ।।

prāya-śaḥ saṃnipātena bhūyasā tūpadiśyate ।
saṃtataḥ satato anye-dyus tṛtīyaka-caturthakau ।।

rāyaḥ sa saṃnipātena
dhātu-mūtra-śakṛd-vāhi-srotasāṃ vyāpino malāḥ ।
tāpayantas tanuṃ sarvāṃ tulya-dūṣyādi-vardhitāḥ ।।

balino guravaḥ stabdhā viśeṣeṇa rasāśritāḥ ।
saṃtataṃ niṣ-prati-dvandvā jvaraṃ kuryuḥ su-duḥ-saham ।।

malaṃ jvaroṣmā dhātūn vā sa śīghraṃ kṣapayet tataḥ ।
sarvākāraṃ rasādīnāṃ śuddhyā-śuddhyāpi vā kramāt ।।

alāñ jvaroṣmā dhātūn vā
vāta-pitta-kaphaiḥ sapta daśa dvā-daśa vāsarān ।
prāyo anuyāti maryādāṃ mokṣāya ca vadhāya ca ।।

imokṣāya vadhāya vā
ity agniveśasya mataṃ hārītasya punaḥ smṛtiḥ ।
dvi-guṇā saptamī yāvan navamy ekā-daśī tathā ।।

eṣā tri-doṣa-maryādā mokṣāya ca vadhāya ca ।
śuddhy-a-śuddhau jvaraḥ kālaṃ dīrgham apy anuvartate ।।

śuddhy-a-śuddhyor jvaraḥ kālaṃ
kṛśānāṃ vyādhi-muktānāṃ mithyāhārādi-sevinām ।
alpo api doṣo dūṣyāder labdhvānya-tamato balam ।।

sa-vipakṣo jvaraṃ kuryād viṣamaṃ kṣaya-vṛddhi-bhāk ।
doṣaḥ pravartate teṣāṃ sve kāle jvarayan balī ।।

va-kāle jvarayan balī
nivartate punaś caiṣa praty-anīka-balā-balaḥ ।
kṣīṇe doṣe jvaraḥ sūkṣmo rasādiṣv eva līyate ।।

līna-tvāt kārśya-vaivarṇya-jāḍyādīn ādadhāti saḥ ।
āsanna-vivṛtāsya-tvāt srotasāṃ rasa-vāhinām ।।

āśu sarvasya vapuṣo vyāptir doṣeṇa jāyate ।
saṃtataḥ satatas tena viparīto viparyayāt ।।

viṣamo viṣamārambha-kriyā-kālo anuṣaṅga-vān ।
doṣo raktāśrayaḥ prāyaḥ karoti satataṃ jvaram ।।

aho-rātrasya sa dviḥ syāt sakṛd anye-dyur āśritaḥ ।
tasmin māṃsa-vahā nāḍīr medo-nāḍīs tṛtīyake ।।

smin māṃsa-vahā nāḍīr
grāhī pittānilān mūrdhnas trikasya kapha-pittataḥ ।
sa-pṛṣṭhasyānila-kaphāt sa caikāhāntaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

a vaikāhāntaraḥ smṛtaḥ
caturthako male medo-majjāsthy-anya-tama-sthite ।
majja-stha evety apare prabhāvaṃ sa tu darśayet ।।

dvi-dhā kaphena jaṅghābhyāṃ sa pūrvaṃ śiraso anilāt ।
asthi-majjobhaya-gate caturthaka-viparyayaḥ ।।

āturthika-viparyayaḥ
tri-dhā dvy-ahaṃ jvarayati dinam ekaṃ tu muñcati ।
balā-balena doṣāṇām anna-ceṣṭādi-janmanā ।।

ry-ahād dvy-ahaṃ jvarayati inam ekaṃ vimuñcati
jvaraḥ syān manasas tad-vat karmaṇaś ca tadā tadā ।
doṣa-dūṣyartv-aho-rātra-prabhṛtīnāṃ balāj jvaraḥ ।।

manaso viṣayāṇāṃ ca kālaṃ taṃ taṃ prapadyate ।
dhātūn prakṣobhayan doṣo mokṣa-kāle vilīyate ।।

tato naraḥ śvasan svidyan kūjan vamati ceṣṭate ।
vepate pralapaty uṣṇaiḥ śītaiś cāṅgair hata-prabhaḥ ।।

vi-saṃjño jvara-vegārtaḥ sa-krodha iva vīkṣate ।
sa-doṣa-śabdaṃ ca śakṛd dravaṃ sṛjati vega-vat ।।

deho laghur vyapagata-klama-moha-tāpaḥ pāko mukhe karaṇa-sauṣṭhavam a-vyatha-tvam । svedaḥ kṣavaḥ prakṛti-yogi mano anna-lipsā kaṇḍūś ca mūrdhni vigata-jvara-lakṣaṇāni ।।

।।

nidānasthāna
bhṛśoṣṇa-tīkṣṇa-kaṭv-amla-lavaṇādi-vidāhibhiḥ ।
kodravoddālakaiś cānnais tad-yuktair ati-sevitaiḥ ।।

kupitaṃ pittalaiḥ pittaṃ dravaṃ raktaṃ ca mūrchite ।
te mithas tulya-rūpa-tvam āgamya vyāpnutas tanum ।।

pittaṃ raktasya vikṛteḥ saṃsargād dūṣaṇād api ।
gandha-varṇānuvṛtteś ca raktena vyapadiśyate ।।

ittaṃ raktasya vikṛtiḥ
prabhavaty asṛjaḥ sthānāt plīhato yakṛtaś ca tat ।
śiro-guru-tvam a-ruciḥ śītecchā dhūmako amlakaḥ ।।

chardiś chardita-baibhatsyaṃ kāsaḥ śvāso bhramaḥ klamaḥ ।
loha-lohita-matsyāma-gandhāsya-tvaṃ svara-kṣayaḥ ।।

rakta-hāridra-harita-varṇa-tā nayanādiṣu ।
nīla-lohita-pītānāṃ varṇānām a-vivecanam ।।

svapne tad-varṇa-darśi-tvaṃ bhavaty asmin bhaviṣyati ।
ūrdhvaṃ nāsākṣi-karṇāsyair meḍhra-yoni-gudair adhaḥ ।।

kupitaṃ roma-kūpaiś ca samastais tat pravartate ।
ūrdhvaṃ sādhyaṃ kaphād yasmāt tad virecana-sādhanam ।।

bahv-auṣadhaṃ ca pittasya vireko hi varauṣadham ।
anubandhī kapho yaś ca tatra tasyāpi śuddhi-kṛt ।।

kaṣāyāḥ svādavo apy asya viśuddha-śleṣmaṇo hitāḥ ।
kim u tiktāḥ kaṣāyā vā ye nisargāt kaphāpahāḥ ।।

adho yāpyaṃ calād yasmāt tat pracchardana-sādhanam ।
alpauṣadhaṃ ca pittasya vamanaṃ na varauṣadham ।।

anubandhī calo yaś ca śāntaye api na tasya tat ।
kaṣāyāś ca hitās tasya madhurā eva kevalam ।।

kapha-māruta-saṃsṛṣṭam a-sādhyam ubhayāyanam ।
a-śakya-prātilomya-tvād a-bhāvād auṣadhasya ca ।।

na hi saṃśodhanaṃ kiñ-cid asty asya pratiloma-gam ।
śodhanaṃ pratilomaṃ ca rakta-pitte bhiṣag-jitam ।।

sty asya pratilomanam sty asya pratilomakam
evam evopaśamanaṃ sarva-śo nāsya vidyate ।
saṃsṛṣṭeṣu hi doṣeṣu sarva-jic chamanaṃ hitam ।।

tatra doṣānugamanaṃ sirāsra iva lakṣayet ।
upadravāṃś ca vikṛti-jñānatas teṣu cādhikam ।।

āśu-kārī yataḥ kāsas tam evātaḥ pravakṣyati ।
pañca kāsāḥ smṛtā vāta-pitta-śleṣma-kṣata-kṣayaiḥ ।।

am evātaḥ pracakṣyate am evātaḥ pracakṣate
kṣayāyopekṣitāḥ sarve balinaś cottarottaram ।
teṣāṃ bhaviṣyatāṃ rūpaṃ kaṇṭhe kaṇḍūr a-rocakaḥ ।।

alinaś ca yathottaram
śūka-pūrṇābha-kaṇṭha-tvaṃ tatrādho vihato anilaḥ ।
ūrdhvaṃ pravṛttaḥ prāpyoras tasmin kaṇṭhe ca saṃsajan ।।

śiraḥ-srotāṃsi saṃpūrya tato aṅgāny utkṣipann iva ।
kṣipann ivākṣiṇī pṛṣṭham uraḥ pārśve ca pīḍayan ।।

pravartate sa vaktreṇa bhinna-kāṃsyopama-dhvaniḥ ।
hetu-bhedāt pratīghāta-bhedo vāyoḥ sa-raṃhasaḥ ।।

yad rujā-śabda-vaiṣamyaṃ kāsānāṃ jāyate tataḥ ।
kupito vātalair vātaḥ śuṣkoraḥ-kaṇṭha-vaktra-tām ।।

upito vātalair vāyuḥ
hṛt-pārśvoraḥ-śiraḥ-śūlaṃ moha-kṣobha-svara-kṣayān ।
karoti śuṣkaṃ kāsaṃ ca mahā-vega-rujā-svanam ।।

aroti śuṣka-kāsaṃ ca
so aṅga-harṣī kaphaṃ śuṣkaṃ kṛcchrān muktvālpa-tāṃ vrajet ।
pittāt pītākṣi-kapha-tā tiktāsya-tvaṃ jvaro bhramaḥ ।।

pittāsṛg-vamanaṃ tṛṣṇā vaisvaryaṃ dhūmako amlakaḥ ।
pratataṃ kāsa-vegena jyotiṣām iva darśanam ।।

aisvaryaṃ dhūmako madaḥ
kaphād uro alpa-ruṅ mūrdha-hṛdayaṃ stimitaṃ guru ।
kaṇṭhopalepaḥ sadanaṃ pīnasa-cchardy-a-rocakāḥ ।।

aṇṭhāsya-lepaḥ sadanaṃ
roma-harṣo ghana-snigdha-śveta-śleṣma-pravartanam ।
yuddhādyaiḥ sāhasais tais taiḥ sevitair a-yathā-balam ।।

urasy antaḥ-kṣate vāyuḥ pittenānugato balī ।
kupitaḥ kurute kāsaṃ kaphaṃ tena sa-śoṇitam ।।

pītaṃ śyāvaṃ ca śuṣkaṃ ca grathitaṃ kuthitaṃ bahu ।
ṣṭhīvet kaṇṭhena rujatā vibhinneneva corasā ।।

ītaṃ śyāmaṃ ca śuṣkaṃ ca
sūcībhir iva tīkṣṇābhis tudyamānena śūlinā ।
parva-bheda-jvara-śvāsa-tṛṣṇā-vaisvarya-kampa-vān ।।

pārāvata ivākūjan pārśva-śūlī tato asya ca ।
kramād vīryaṃ ruciḥ paktā balaṃ varṇaś ca hīyate ।।

kṣīṇasya sāsṛṅ-mūtra-tvaṃ syāc ca pṛṣṭha-kaṭī-grahaḥ ।
vāyu-pradhānāḥ kupitā dhātavo rāja-yakṣmiṇaḥ ।।

kurvanti yakṣmāyatanaiḥ kāsaṃ ṣṭhīvet kaphaṃ tataḥ ।
pūti-pūyopamaṃ pītaṃ visraṃ harita-lohitam ।।

lucyete iva pārśve ca hṛdayaṃ patatīva ca ।
a-kasmād uṣṇa-śītecchā bahv-āśi-tvaṃ bala-kṣayaḥ ।।

upyete iva pārśve ca
snigdha-prasanna-vaktra-tvaṃ śrī-mad-darśana-netra-tā ।
tato asya kṣaya-rūpāṇi sarvāṇy āvir-bhavanti ca ।।

śrī-mad-daśana-netra-tā
ity eṣa kṣaya-jaḥ kāsaḥ kṣīṇānāṃ deha-nāśanaḥ ।
yāpyo vā balināṃ tad-vat kṣata-jo abhinavau tu tau ।।

sidhyetām api sānāthyāt sādhyā doṣaiḥ pṛthak trayaḥ ।
miśrā yāpyā dvayāt sarve jarasā sthavirasya ca ।।

idhyetām api sāmarthyāt
kāsāc chvāsa-kṣaya-cchardi-svara-sādādayo gadāḥ ।
bhavanty upekṣayā yasmāt tasmāt taṃ tvarayā jayet ।।

nidānasthāna
kāsa-vṛddhyā bhavec chvāsaḥ pūrvair vā doṣa-kopanaiḥ ।
āmātīsāra-vamathu-viṣa-pāṇḍu-jvarair api ।।

rajo-dhūmānilair marma-ghātād ati-himāmbunā ।
kṣudrakas tamakaś chinno mahān ūrdhvaś ca pañcamaḥ ।।

kaphoparuddha-gamanaḥ pavano viṣvag-āsthitaḥ ।
prāṇodakānna-vāhīni duṣṭaḥ srotāṃsi dūṣayan ।।

uraḥ-sthaḥ kurute śvāsam āmāśaya-samudbhavam ।
prāg-rūpaṃ tasya hṛt-pārśva-śūlaṃ prāṇa-viloma-tā ।।

ānāhaḥ śaṅkha-bhedaś ca tatrāyāsāti-bhojanaiḥ ।
preritaḥ prerayet kṣudraṃ svayaṃ saṃśamanaṃ marut ।।

pratilomaṃ sirā gacchann udīrya pavanaḥ kapham ।
parigṛhya śiro-grīvam uraḥ pārśve ca pīḍayan ।।

kāsaṃ ghurghurakaṃ moham a-rucim pīnasaṃ tṛṣam ।
karoti tīvra-vegaṃ ca śvāsaṃ prāṇopatāpinam ।।

pratāmyet tasya vegena niṣṭhyūtānte kṣaṇaṃ sukhī ।
kṛcchrāc chayānaḥ śvasiti niṣaṇṇaḥ svāsthyam ṛcchati ।।

ucchritākṣo lalāṭena svidyatā bhṛśam arti-mān ।
viśuṣkāsyo muhuḥ-śvāsī kāṅkṣaty uṣṇaṃ sa-vepathuḥ ।।

meghāmbu-śīta-prāg-vātaiḥ śleṣmalaiś ca vivardhate ।
sa yāpyas tamako sādhyo navo vā balino bhavet ।।

jvara-mūrchā-yutaḥ śītaiḥ śāmyet pratamakas tu saḥ ।
chinnāc chvasiti vicchinnaṃ marma-ccheda-rujārditaḥ ।।

sa-sveda-mūrchaḥ sānāho vasti-dāha-nirodha-vān ।
adho-dṛg viplutākṣaś ca muhyan raktaika-locanaḥ ।।

śuṣkāsyaḥ pralapan dīno naṣṭa-cchāyo vi-cetanaḥ ।
mahatā mahatā dīno nādena śvasiti krathan ।।

ahato mahatā dīno
uddhūyamānaḥ saṃrabdho mattarṣabha ivā-niśam ।
praṇaṣṭa-jñāna-vijñāno vibhrānta-nayanānanaḥ ।।

vakṣaḥ samākṣipan baddha-mūtra-varcā viśīrṇa-vāk ।
śuṣka-kaṇṭho muhur muhyan karṇa-śaṅkha-śiro-'ti-ruk ।।

dīrgham ūrdhvaṃ śvasity ūrdhvān na ca pratyāharaty adhaḥ ।
śleṣmāvṛta-mukha-srotāḥ kruddha-gandha-vahārditaḥ ।।

ūrdhva-dṛg vīkṣate bhrāntam akṣiṇī paritaḥ kṣipan ।
marmasu cchidyamāneṣu paridevī niruddha-vāk ।।

ete sidhyeyur a-vyaktā vyaktāḥ prāṇa-harā dhruvam ।
śvāsaika-hetu-prāg-rūpa-saṃkhyā-prakṛti-saṃśrayāḥ ।।

-saṃkhyā-prakṛti-saṃśrayā
hidhmā bhaktodbhavā kṣudrā yamalā mahatīti ca ।
gambhīrā ca marut tatra tvarayā-yukti-sevitaiḥ ।।

rūkṣa-tīkṣṇa-kharā-sātmyair anna-pānaiḥ prapīḍitaḥ ।
karoti hidhmām a-rujāṃ manda-śabdāṃ kṣavānugām ।।

śamaṃ sātmyānna-pānena yā prayāti ca sānna-jā ।
āyāsāt pavanaḥ kṣudraḥ kṣudrāṃ hidhmāṃ pravartayet ।।

āyāsāt pavanaḥ kruddhaḥ
jatru-mūla-pravisṛtām alpa-vegāṃ mṛduṃ ca sā ।
vṛddhim āyāsyato yāti bhukta-mātre ca mārdavam ।।

cireṇa yamalair vegair āhāre yā pravartate ।
pariṇāmon-mukhe vṛddhiṃ pariṇāme ca gacchati ।।

kampayantī śiro-grīvam ādhmātasyāti-tṛṣyataḥ ।
pralāpa-cchardy-atīsāra-netra-vipluti-jṛmbhiṇaḥ ।।

ampayantī śiro-grīvām
yamalā veginī hidhmā pariṇāma-vatī ca sā ।
stabdha-bhrū-śaṅkha-yugmasya sāsra-vipluta-cakṣuṣaḥ ।।

hvasta-bhrū-śaṅkha-yugmasya āśru-vipluta-cakṣuṣaḥ
stambhayantī tanuṃ vācaṃ smṛtiṃ saṃjñāṃ ca muṣṇatī ।
rundhatī mārgam annasya kurvatī marma-ghaṭṭanam ।।

pṛṣṭhato namanaṃ śoṣaṃ mahā-hidhmā pravartate ।
mahā-mūlā mahā-śabdā mahā-vegā mahā-balā ।।

pakvāśayād vā nābher vā pūrva-vad yā pravartate ।
tad-rūpā sā muhuḥ kuryāj jṛmbhām aṅga-prasāraṇam ।।

gambhīreṇānunādena gambhīrā tāsu sādhayet ।
ādye dve varjayed antye sarva-liṅgāṃ ca veginīm ।।

sarvāś ca saṃcitāmasya sthavirasya vyavāyinaḥ ।
vyādhibhiḥ kṣīṇa-dehasya bhakta-ccheda-kṣatasya vā ।।

sarve api rogā nāśāya na tv evaṃ śīghra-kāriṇaḥ ।
hidhmā-śvāsau yathā tau hi mṛtyu-kāle kṛtālayau ।।

nidānasthāna
aneka-rogānugato bahu-roga-puro-gamaḥ ।
rāja-yakṣmā kṣayaḥ śoṣo roga-rāḍ iti ca smṛtaḥ ।।

nakṣatrāṇāṃ dvi-jānāṃ ca rājño abhūd yad ayaṃ purā ।
yac ca rājā ca yakṣmā ca rāja-yakṣmā tato mataḥ ।।

dehauṣadha-kṣaya-kṛteḥ kṣayas tat-saṃbhavāc ca saḥ ।
rasādi-śoṣaṇāc choṣo roga-rāṭ teṣu rājanāt ।।

oga-rāṭ roga-rājanāt
sāhasaṃ vega-saṃrodhaḥ śukraujaḥ-sneha-saṃkṣayaḥ ।
anna-pāna-vidhi-tyāgaś catvāras tasya hetavaḥ ।।

tair udīrṇo anilaḥ pittaṃ kaphaṃ codīrya sarvataḥ ।
śarīra-saṃdhīn āviśya tān sirāś ca prapīḍayan ।।

mukhāni srotasāṃ ruddhvā tathaivātivivṛtya vā ।
sarpann ūrdhvam adhas tiryag yathā-svaṃ janayed gadān ।।

rūpaṃ bhaviṣyatas tasya pratiśyāyo bhṛśaṃ kṣavaḥ ।
praseko mukha-mādhuryaṃ sadanaṃ vahni-dehayoḥ ।।

sthāly-amatrānna-pānādau śucāv apy a-śucīkṣaṇam ।
makṣikā-tṛṇa-keśādi-pātaḥ prāyo anna-pānayoḥ ।।

hṛl-lāsaś chardir a-rucir aśnato api bala-kṣayaḥ ।
pāṇyor avekṣā pādāsya-śopho akṣṇor ati-śukla-tā ।।

bāhvoḥ pramāṇa-jijñāsā kāye baibhatsya-darśanam ।
strī-madya-māṃsa-priya-tā ghṛṇi-tvaṃ mūrdha-guṇṭhanam ।।

nakha-keśāti-vṛddhiś ca svapne cābhibhavo bhavet ।
pataṅga-kṛkalāsāhi-kapi-śvāpada-pakṣibhiḥ ।।

-kapi-śvāpada-pattribhiḥ
keśāsthi-tuṣa-bhasmādi-rāśau samadhirohaṇam ।
śūnyānāṃ grāma-deśānāṃ darśanaṃ śuṣyato ambhaso ।।

jyotir girīṇāṃ patatāṃ jvalatāṃ ca mahī-ruhām ।
pīnasa-śvāsa-kāsāṃsa-mūrdha-svara-rujo a-ruciḥ ।।

ūrdhvaṃ viḍ-bhraṃśa-saṃśoṣāv adhaś chardiś ca koṣṭha-ge ।
tiryak-sthe pārśva-rug-doṣe saṃdhi-ge bhavati jvaraḥ ।।

ūrdhvaṃ viṭ-sraṃsa-saṃśoṣāv dhaś chardis tu koṣṭha-ge
rūpāṇy ekā-daśaitāni jāyante rāja-yakṣmiṇaḥ ।
teṣām upadravān vidyāt kaṇṭhoddhvaṃsam uro-rujam ।।

jṛmbhāṅga-marda-niṣṭhīva-vahni-sādāsya-pūti-tāḥ ।
tatra vātāc chiraḥ-pārśva-śūlam aṃsāṅga-mardanam ।।

kaṇṭhoddhvaṃsaḥ svara-bhraṃśaḥ pittāt pādāṃsa-pāṇiṣu ।
dāho atīsāro asṛk-chardir mukha-gandho jvaro madaḥ ।।

kaphād a-rocakaś chardiḥ kāso mūrdhāṅga-gauravam ।
prasekaḥ pīnasaḥ śvāsaḥ svara-sādo alpa-vahni-tā ।।

vara-bhedo alpa-vahni-tā
doṣair mandānala-tvena sopalepaiḥ kapholbaṇaiḥ ।
sroto-mukheṣu ruddheṣu dhātūṣmasv alpakeṣu ca ।।

vidahyamānaḥ sva-sthāne rasas tāṃs tān upadravān ।
kuryād a-gacchan māṃsādīn asṛk cordhvaṃ pradhāvati ।।

pacyate koṣṭha evānnam anna-paktraiva cāsya yat ।
prāyo asmān mala-tāṃ yātaṃ naivālaṃ dhātu-puṣṭaye ।।

raso apy asya na raktāya māṃsāya kuta eva tu ।
upastabdhaḥ sa śakṛtā kevalaṃ vartate kṣayī ।।

paṣṭabdhaḥ sa śakṛtā
liṅgeṣv alpeṣv api kṣīṇaṃ vyādhy-auṣadha-balā-kṣamam ।
varjayet sādhayed eva sarveṣv api tato anya-thā ।।

arjayet sādhayed evaṃ
kṣīṇa-māṃsa-balaṃ jahyāt pūrva-liṅgair upadrutam ।
pratyākhyāya naraṃ cāśu dravya-vantam upācaret ।।

doṣair vyastaiḥ samastaiś ca kṣayāt ṣaṣṭhaś ca medasā ।
svara-bhedo bhavet tatra kṣāmo rūkṣaś calaḥ svaraḥ ।।

ṣayāt ṣaṣṭhaś ca medasaḥ
śūka-pūrṇābha-kaṇṭha-tvaṃ snigdhoṣṇopaśayo anilāt ।
pittāt tālu-gale dāhaḥ śoṣa uktāvasūyanam ।।

limpann iva kaphāt kaṇṭhaṃ mandaḥ khurakhurāyate ।
svaro vibaddhaḥ sarvais tu sarva-liṅgaḥ kṣayāt kaṣet ।।

dhūmāyatīva cāty-arthaṃ medasā śleṣma-lakṣaṇaḥ ।
kṛcchra-lakṣyākṣaraś cātra sarvair antyaṃ ca varjayet ।।

a-rocako bhaved doṣair jihvā-hṛdaya-saṃśrayaiḥ ।
saṃnipātena manasaḥ saṃtāpena ca pañcamaḥ ।।

ihvā-hṛdaya-saṃśritaiḥ
kaṣāya-tikta-madhuraṃ vātādiṣu mukhaṃ kramāt ।
sarvotthe vi-rasaṃ śoka-krodhādiṣu yathā-malam ।।

chardir doṣaiḥ pṛthak sarvair dviṣṭair arthaiś ca pañcamī ।
udāno vikṛto doṣān sarvāsv apy ūrdhvam asyati ।।

tāsūtkleśāsya-lāvaṇya-prasekā-rucayo agra-gāḥ ।
nābhi-pṛṣṭhaṃ rujan vāyuḥ pārśve cāhāram utkṣipet ।।

tato vicchinnam alpālpaṃ kaṣāyaṃ phenilaṃ vamet ।
śabdodgāra-yutaṃ kṛṣṇam acchaṃ kṛcchreṇa vega-vat ।।

kāsāsya-śoṣa-hṛn-mūrdha-svara-pīḍā-klamānvitaḥ ।
pittāt kṣārodaka-nibhaṃ dhūmraṃ harita-pītakam ।।

sāsṛg amlaṃ kaṭūṣṇaṃ ca tṛṇ-mūrchā-tāpa-dāha-vat ।
kaphāt snigdhaṃ ghanaṃ śītaṃ śleṣma-tantu-gavākṣitam ।।

ṛṇ-mūrchā-tāpa-dāha-vān
madhuraṃ lavaṇaṃ bhūri prasaktaṃ roma-harṣaṇam ।
mukha-śvayathu-mādhurya-tandrā-hṛl-lāsa-kāsa-vān ।।

sarva-liṅgā malaiḥ sarvai riṣṭoktā yā ca tāṃ tyajet ।
pūty-a-medhyā-śuci-dviṣṭa-darśana-śravaṇādibhiḥ ।।

tapte citte hṛdi kliṣṭe chardir dviṣṭārtha-yoga-jā ।
vātādīn eva vimṛśet kṛmi-tṛṇāma-daurhṛde ।।

śūla-vepathu-hṛl-lāsair viśeṣāt kṛmi-jāṃ vadet ।
kṛmi-hṛd-roga-liṅgaiś ca smṛtāḥ pañca tu hṛd-gadāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ gulma-nidānoktaiḥ samutthānaiś ca saṃbhavaḥ ।
vātena śūlyate aty-arthaṃ tudyate sphuṭatīva ca ।।

amutthānaiḥ samudbhavaḥ
bhidyate śuṣyati stabdhaṃ hṛdayaṃ śūnya-tā dravaḥ ।
a-kasmād dīna-tā śoko bhayaṃ śabdā-sahiṣṇu-tā ।।

ṛdayaṃ śūnya-tā-dravam
vepathur veṣṭanaṃ mohaḥ śvāsa-rodho alpa-nidra-tā ।
pittāt tṛṣṇā bhramo mūrchā dāhaḥ svedo amlakaḥ klamaḥ ।।

chardanaṃ cāmla-pittasya dhūmakaḥ pīta-tā jvaraḥ ।
śleṣmaṇā hṛdayaṃ stabdhaṃ bhārikaṃ sāśma-garbha-vat ।।

amakaḥ pīta-tā jvaraḥ
kāsāgni-sāda-niṣṭhīva-nidrālasyā-ruci-jvarāḥ ।
sarva-liṅgas tribhir doṣaiḥ kṛmibhiḥ śyāva-netra-tā ।।

arva-liṅgaṃ tribhir doṣaiḥ
tamaḥ-praveśo hṛl-lāsaḥ śoṣaḥ kaṇḍūḥ kapha-srutiḥ ।
hṛdayaṃ pratataṃ cātra krakaceneva dāryate ।।

cikitsed āmayaṃ ghoraṃ taṃ śīghraṃ śīghra-kāriṇam ।
vātāt pittāt kaphāt tṛṣṇā saṃnipātād rasa-kṣayāt ।।

ṣaṣṭhī syād upasargāc ca vāta-pitte tu kāraṇam ।
sarvāsu tat-prakopo hi saumya-dhātu-praśoṣaṇāt ।।

sarva-deha-bhramotkampa-tāpa-tṛḍ-dāha-moha-kṛt ।
jihvā-mūla-gala-kloma-tālu-toya-vahāḥ sirāḥ ।।

saṃśoṣya tṛṣṇā jāyante tāsāṃ sāmānya-lakṣaṇam ।
mukha-śoṣo jalā-tṛptir anna-dveṣaḥ svara-kṣayaḥ ।।

kaṇṭhauṣṭha-jihvā-kārkaśyaṃ jihvā-niṣkramaṇaṃ klamaḥ ।
pralāpaś citta-vibhraṃśas tṛḍ-grahoktās tathāmayāḥ ।।

mārutāt kṣāma-tā dainyaṃ śaṅkha-todaḥ śiro-bhramaḥ ।
gandhā-jñānāsya-vairasya-śruti-nidrā-bala-kṣayāḥ ।।

andhā-jñānāsya-vairasyaṃ -śruti-nidrā-bala-kṣayaḥ 
śruti-nidrā-bala-kṣayaḥ
śītāmbu-pānād vṛddhiś ca pittān mūrchāsya-tikta-tā ।
raktekṣaṇa-tvaṃ pratataṃ śoṣo dāho ati-dhūmakaḥ ।।

kapho ruṇaddhi kupitas toya-vāhiṣu mārutam ।
srotaḥsu sa kaphas tena paṅka-vac choṣyate tataḥ ।।

śūkair ivācitaḥ kaṇṭho nidrā madhura-vaktra-tā ।
ādhmānaṃ śiraso jāḍyaṃ staimitya-cchardy-a-rocakāḥ ।।

ālasyam a-vipākaś ca sarvaiḥ syāt sarva-lakṣaṇā ।
āmodbhavā ca bhaktasya saṃrodhād vāta-pitta-jā ।।

uṣṇa-klāntasya sahasā śītāmbho bhajatas tṛṣam ।
ūṣmā ruddho gataḥ koṣṭhaṃ yāṃ kuryāt pitta-jaiva sā ।।

yā ca pānāti-pānotthā tīkṣṇāgneḥ sneha-jā ca yā ।
snigdha-gurv-amla-lavaṇa-bhojanena kaphodbhavā ।।

īkṣṇāgni-sneha-jā ca yā
tṛṣṇā rasa-kṣayoktena lakṣaṇena kṣayātmikā ।
śoṣa-meha-jvarādy-anya-dīrgha-rogopasargataḥ ।।

śoṣa-moha-jvarādy-anya- yā tṛṣṇā jāyate tīvrā sopasargātmikā smṛtā ।।

nidānasthāna
tīkṣṇoṣṇa-rūkṣa-sūkṣmāmlaṃ vyavāyy āśu-karaṃ laghu ।
vikāṣi viśadaṃ madyam ojaso asmād viparyayaḥ ।।

īkṣṇoṣṇa-rūkṣa-sūkṣmāmla- -vyavāyy āśu-karaṃ laghu 
vikāśi viśadaṃ madyam
tīkṣṇādayo viṣe apy uktāś cittopaplāvino guṇāḥ ।
jīvitāntāya jāyante viṣe tūtkarṣa-vṛttitaḥ ।।

tīkṣṇādibhir guṇair madyaṃ mandādīn ojaso guṇān ।
daśabhir daśa saṃkṣobhya ceto nayati vi-kriyām ।।

ādye made dvitīye tu pramādāyatane sthitaḥ ।
dur-vikalpa-hato mūḍhaḥ sukham ity adhimucyate ।।

ādye made dvitīye ca ādye made dvitīye sa ukham ity abhimucyate 
ukham ity abhimanyate ukham ity avamanyate
madhyamottamayoḥ saṃdhiṃ prāpya rājasa-tāmasaḥ ।
nir-aṅkuśa iva vyālo na kiñ-cin nācarej jaḍaḥ ।।

a kiṃ kiṃ vācarej jaḍaḥ
iyaṃ bhūmir a-vadyānāṃ dauḥśīlyasyedam āspadam ।
eko ayaṃ bahu-mārgāya dur-gater deśikaḥ param ।।

yaṃ bhūmir a-vidyānāṃ
niś-ceṣṭaḥ śava-vac chete tṛtīye tu made sthitaḥ ।
maraṇād api pāpātmā gataḥ pāpa-tarāṃ daśām ।।

dharmā-dharmaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkham arthān-arthaṃ hitā-hitam ।
yad āsakto na jānāti kathaṃ tac chīlayed budhaḥ ।।

madye moho bhayaṃ śokaḥ krodho mṛtyuś ca saṃśritāḥ ।
sonmāda-mada-mūrchāyāḥ sāpasmārāpatānakāḥ ।।

yatraikaḥ smṛti-vibhraṃśas tatra sarvam a-sādhu yat ।
a-yukti-yuktam annaṃ hi vyādhaye maraṇāya vā ।।

madyaṃ tri-varga-dhī-dhairya-lajjāder api nāśanam ।
nātimādyanti balinaḥ kṛtāhārā mahāśanāḥ ।।

snigdhāḥ sat-tva-vayo-yuktā madya-nityās tad-anvayāḥ ।
medaḥ-kaphādhikā manda-vāta-pittā dṛḍhāgnayaḥ ।।

viparyaye atimādyanti viśrabdhāḥ kupitāś ca ye ।
madyena cāmla-rūkṣeṇa sā-jīrṇe bahunāti ca ।।

ā-jīrṇe bahunāpi ca
vātāt pittāt kaphāt sarvaiś catvāraḥ syur madātyayāḥ ।
sarve api sarvair jāyante vyapadeśas tu bhūyasā ।।

sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ teṣāṃ pramoho hṛdaya-vyathā ।
viḍ-bhedaḥ pratataṃ tṛṣṇā saumyāgneyo jvaro a-ruciḥ ।।

ramoho hṛdaye vyathā
śiraḥ-pārśvāsthi-ruk-kampo marma-bhedas trika-grahaḥ ।
uro-vibandhas timiraṃ kāsaḥ śvāsaḥ prajāgaraḥ ।।

śiraḥ-pārśvāsthi-ruk-stambho
svedo ati-mātraṃ viṣṭambhaḥ śvayathuś citta-vibhramaḥ ।
pralāpaś chardir utkleśo bhramo duḥ-svapna-darśanam ।।

viśeṣāj jāgara-śvāsa-kampa-mūrdha-rujo anilāt ।
svapne bhramaty utpatati pretaiś ca saha bhāṣate ।।

pittād dāha-jvara-sveda-mohātīsāra-tṛḍ-bhramāḥ ।
deho harita-hāridro rakta-netra-kapola-tā ।।

śleṣmaṇā chardi-hṛl-lāsa-nidrodardāṅga-gauravam ।
sarva-je sarva-liṅga-tvaṃ muktvā madyaṃ pibet tu yaḥ ।।

śleṣmaṇaś chardi-hṛl-lāsa-
sahasān-ucitaṃ vānyat tasya dhvaṃsaka-vikṣayau ।
bhavetāṃ mārutāt kaṣṭau dur-balasya viśeṣataḥ ।।

ahasān-ucitaṃ cānyat asya dhvaṃsaka-viṭ-kṣayau
dhvaṃsake śleṣma-niṣṭhīvaḥ kaṇṭha-śoṣo ati-nidra-tā ।
śabdā-saha-tvaṃ tandrā ca vikṣaye aṅga-śiro-'ti-ruk ।।

iṭ-kṣaye aṅga-śiro-'ti-ruk
hṛt-kaṇṭha-rogaḥ saṃmohaḥ kāsas tṛṣṇā vamir jvaraḥ ।
nivṛtto yas tu madyebhyo jitātmā buddhi-pūrva-kṛt ।।

ṛt-kaṇṭha-rodhaḥ saṃmohaḥ
vikāraiḥ spṛśyate jātu na sa śārīra-mānasaiḥ ।
rajo-mohā-hitāhāra-parasya syus trayo gadāḥ ।।

rasāsṛk-cetanā-vāhi-sroto-rodha-samudbhavāḥ ।
mada-mūrchāya-saṃnyāsā yathottara-balottarāḥ ।।

mado atra doṣaiḥ sarvaiś ca rakta-madya-viṣair api ।
saktān-alpa-drutābhāṣaś calaḥ skhalita-ceṣṭitaḥ ।।

rūkṣa-śyāvāruṇa-tanur made vātodbhave bhavet ।
pittena krodhano rakta-pītābhaḥ kalaha-priyaḥ ।।

ade vāta-kṛte bhavet
sv-alpa-saṃbaddha-vāk pāṇḍuḥ kaphād dhyāna-paro alasaḥ ।
sarvātmā saṃnipātena raktāt stabdhāṅga-dṛṣṭi-tā ।।

v-alpā-saṃbaddha-vāk pāṇḍuḥ
pitta-liṅgaṃ ca madyena vikṛteha-svarāṅga-tā ।
viṣe kampo ati-nidrā ca sarvebhyo abhyadhikas tu saḥ ।।

iṣāt kampo ati-nidrā ca arvebhyo abhyadhikaś ca saḥ
lakṣayel lakṣaṇotkarṣād vātādīn śoṇitādiṣu ।
aruṇaṃ kṛṣṇa-nīlaṃ vā khaṃ paśyan praviśet tamaḥ ।।

śīghraṃ ca pratibudhyeta hṛt-pīḍā vepathur bhramaḥ ।
kārśyaṃ śyāvāruṇā chāyā mūrchāye mārutātmake ।।

ārśyaṃ śyāvāruṇa-cchāye
pittena raktaṃ pītaṃ vā nabhaḥ paśyan viśet tamaḥ ।
vibudhyeta ca sa-svedo dāha-tṛṭ-tāpa-pīḍitaḥ ।।

bhinna-viṇ nīla-pītābho rakta-pītākulekṣaṇaḥ ।
kaphena megha-saṃkāśaṃ paśyann ākāśam āviśet ।।

tamaś cirāc ca budhyeta sa-hṛl-lāsaḥ praseka-vān ।
gurubhiḥ stimitair aṅgair ārdra-carmāvanaddha-vat ।।

sarvākṛtis tribhir doṣair apasmāra ivāparaḥ ।
pātayaty āśu niś-ceṣṭaṃ vinā bībhatsa-ceṣṭitaiḥ ।।

inā baibhatsya-ceṣṭitaiḥ
doṣeṣu mada-mūrchāyāḥ kṛta-vegeṣu dehinām ।
svayam evopaśāmyanti saṃnyāso nauṣadhair vinā ।।

vāg-deha-manasāṃ ceṣṭām ākṣipyāti-balā malāḥ ।
saṃnyāsaṃ saṃnipatitāḥ prāṇāyatana-saṃśrayāḥ ।।

kurvanti tena puruṣaḥ kāṣṭhī-bhūto mṛtopamaḥ ।
mriyeta śīghraṃ śīghraṃ cec cikitsā na prayujyate ।।

āṣṭha-bhūto mṛtopamaḥ
a-gādhe grāha-bahule salilaugha ivāṭate ।
saṃnyāse vinimajjantaṃ naram āśu nivartayet ।।

bhinyāse ca majjantaṃ
mada-māna-roṣa-toṣa-prabhṛtibhir aribhir nijaiḥ pariṣvaṅgaḥ ।
yuktā-yuktaṃ ca samaṃ yukti-viyuktena madyena ।।

bala-kāla-deśa-sātmya-prakṛti-sahāyāmaya-vayāṃsi ।
pravibhajya tad-anurūpaṃ yadi pibati tataḥ pibaty amṛtam ।।

nidānasthāna
ari-vat prāṇino māṃsa-kīlakā viśasanti yat ।
arśāṃsi tasmād ucyante guda-mārga-nirodhataḥ ।।

doṣās tvaṅ-māṃsa-medāṃsi saṃdūṣya vividhākṛtīn ।
māṃsāṅkurān apānādau kurvanty arśāṃsi tān jaguḥ ।।

saha-janmottarotthāna-bhedād dve-dhā samāsataḥ ।
śuṣka-srāvi-vibhedāc ca gudaḥ sthūlāntra-saṃśrayaḥ ।।

ardha-pañcāṅgulas tasmiṃs tisro adhy-ardhāṅgulāḥ sthitāḥ ।
balyaḥ pravāhiṇī tāsām antar madhye visarjanī ।।

bāhyā saṃvaraṇī tasyā gudauṣṭho bahir aṅgule ।
yavādhy-ardhaḥ pramāṇena romāṇy atra tataḥ param ।।

āhyā saṃvaraṇī tasyāṃ avādhy-ardha-pramāṇena
tatra hetuḥ sahotthānāṃ valī-bījopatapta-tā ।
arśasāṃ bīja-taptis tu mātā-pitr-apacārataḥ ।।

alī-bījopatapti-tā
daivāc ca tābhyāṃ kopo hi saṃnipātasya tāny ataḥ ।
a-sādhyāny evam ākhyātāḥ sarve rogāḥ kulodbhavāḥ ।।

saha-jāni viśeṣeṇa rūkṣa-dur-darśanāni ca ।
antar-mukhāni pāṇḍūni dāruṇopadravāṇi ca ।।

ṣo-ḍhānyāni pṛthag doṣa-saṃsarga-nicayāsrataḥ ।
śuṣkāṇi vāta-śleṣmabhyām ārdrāṇi tv asra-pittataḥ ।।

doṣa-prakopa-hetus tu prāg uktas tena sādite ।
agnau male ati-nicite punaś cāti-vyavāyataḥ ।।

yāna-saṃkṣobha-viṣama-kaṭhinotkaṭakāsanāt ।
vasti-netrāśma-loṣṭorvī-tala-cailādi-ghaṭṭanāt ।।

bhṛśaṃ śītāmbu-saṃsparśāt pratatāti-pravāhaṇāt ।
vāta-mūtra-śakṛd-vega-dhāraṇāt tad-udīraṇāt ।।

jvara-gulmātisārāma-grahaṇī-śopha-pāṇḍubhiḥ ।
karśanād viṣamābhyaś ca ceṣṭābhyo yoṣitāṃ punaḥ ।।

āma-garbha-prapatanād garbha-vṛddhi-prapīḍanāt ।
īdṛśaiś cāparair vāyur apānaḥ kupito malam ।।

pāyor valīṣu taṃ dhatte tāsv abhiṣyaṇṇa-mūrtiṣu ।
jāyante arśāṃsi tat-pūrva-lakṣaṇaṃ manda-vahni-tā ।।

āyu-valīṣu taṃ dhatte āyor valīṣu saṃdhatte
viṣṭambhaḥ sakthi-sadanaṃ piṇḍikodveṣṭanaṃ bhramaḥ ।
sādo aṅge netrayoḥ śophaḥ śakṛd-bhedo atha-vā grahaḥ ।।

mārutaḥ pracuro mūḍhaḥ prāyo nābher adhaś caran ।
sa-ruk sa-parikartaś ca kṛcchrān nirgacchati svanam ।।

antra-kūjanam āṭopaḥ kṣāma-todgāra-bhūri-tā ।
prabhūtaṃ mūtram alpā viḍ a-śraddhā dhūmako amlakaḥ ।।

rabhūta-mūtra-tālpā viḍ
śiraḥ-pṛṣṭhorasāṃ śūlam ālasyaṃ bhinna-varṇa-tā ।
tandrendriyāṇāṃ daurbalyaṃ krodho duḥkhopacāra-tā ।।

āśaṅkā grahaṇī-doṣa-pāṇḍu-gulmodareṣu ca ।
etāny eva vivardhante jāteṣu hata-nāmasu ।।

tāny eva ca vardhante
nivartamāno apāno hi tair adho-mārga-rodhataḥ ।
kṣobhayann anilān anyān sarvendriya-śarīra-gān ।।

tathā mūtra-śakṛt-pitta-kaphān dhātūṃś ca sāśayān ।
mṛdnāty agniṃ tataḥ sarvo bhavati prāya-śo arśasaḥ ।।

kṛśo bhṛśaṃ hatotsāho dīnaḥ kṣāmo ati-niṣ-prabhaḥ ।
a-sāro vigata-cchāyo jantu-juṣṭa iva drumaḥ ।।

kṛtsnair upadravair grasto yathoktair marma-pīḍanaiḥ ।
tathā kāsa-pipāsāsya-vairasya-śvāsa-pīnasaiḥ ।।

klamāṅga-bhaṅga-vamathu-kṣavathu-śvayathu-jvaraiḥ ।
klaibya-bādhirya-taimirya-śarkarāśmari-pīḍitaḥ ।।

kṣāma-bhinna-svaro dhyāyan muhuḥ ṣṭhīvan a-rocakī ।
sarva-parvāsthi-hṛn-nābhi-pāyu-vaṅkṣaṇa-śūla-vān ।।

gudena sravatā picchāṃ pulākodaka-saṃnibhām ।
vibaddha-muktaṃ śuṣkārdraṃ pakvāmaṃ cāntarāntarā ।।

pāṇḍu pītaṃ harid raktaṃ picchilaṃ copaveśyate ।
gudāṅkurā bahv-anilāḥ śuṣkāś cimicimānvitāḥ ।।

mlānāḥ śyāvāruṇāḥ stabdhā viṣamāḥ paruṣāḥ kharāḥ ।
mitho vi-sadṛśā vakrās tīkṣṇā visphuṭitānanāḥ ।।

bimbī-karkandhu-kharjūra-kārpāsī-phala-saṃnibhāḥ ।
ke-cit kadamba-puṣpābhāḥ ke-cit siddhārthakopamāḥ ।।

śiraḥ-pārśvāṃsa-kaṭy-ūru-vaṅkṣaṇābhyadhika-vyathāḥ ।
kṣavathūdgāra-viṣṭambha-hṛd-grahā-rocaka-pradāḥ ।।

-hṛd-ravā-rocaka-pradāḥ
kāsa-śvāsāgni-vaiṣamya-karṇa-nāda-bhramāvahāḥ ।
tair ārto grathitaṃ stokaṃ sa-śabdaṃ sa-pravāhikam ।।

ruk-phena-picchānugataṃ vibaddham upaveśyate ।
kṛṣṇa-tvaṅ-nakha-viṇ-mūtra-netra-vaktraś ca jāyate ।।

gulma-plīhodarāṣṭhīlā-saṃbhavas tata eva ca ।
pittottarā nīla-mukhā rakta-pītāsita-prabhāḥ ।।

tanv-asra-srāviṇo visrās tanavo mṛdavaḥ ślathāḥ ।
śuka-jihvā-yakṛt-khaṇḍa-jalauko-vaktra-saṃnibhāḥ ।।

dāha-pāka-jvara-sveda-tṛṇ-mūrchā-ruci-moha-dāḥ ।
soṣmāṇo drava-nīloṣṇa-pīta-raktāma-varcasaḥ ।।

yava-madhyā harit-pīta-hāridra-tvaṅ-nakhādayaḥ ।
śleṣmolbaṇā mahā-mūlā ghanā manda-rujaḥ sitāḥ ।।

ava-madhyā harit-pītā āridra-tvaṅ-nakhādayaḥ
ucchūnopācitāḥ snigdhāḥ stabdha-vṛtta-guru-sthirāḥ ।
picchilāḥ stimitāḥ ślakṣṇāḥ kaṇḍv-āḍhyāḥ sparśana-priyāḥ ।।

karīra-panasāsthy-ābhās tathā go-stana-saṃnibhāḥ ।
vaṅkṣaṇānāhinaḥ pāyu-vasti-nābhi-vikartinaḥ ।।

sa-kāsa-śvāsa-hṛl-lāsa-prasekā-ruci-pīnasāḥ ।
meha-kṛcchra-śiro-jāḍya-śiśira-jvara-kāriṇaḥ ।।

klaibyāgni-mārdava-cchardir-āma-prāya-vikāra-dāḥ ।
vasābha-sa-kapha-prājya-purīṣāḥ sa-pravāhikāḥ ।।

asābhāḥ sa-kapha-prājya-
na sravanti na bhidyante pāṇḍu-snigdha-tvag-ādayaḥ ।
saṃsṛṣṭa-liṅgāḥ saṃsargān nicayāt sarva-lakṣaṇāḥ ।।

raktolbaṇā gude-kīlāḥ pittākṛti-samanvitāḥ ।
vaṭa-praroha-sadṛśā guñjā-vidruma-saṃnibhāḥ ।।

te aty-arthaṃ duṣṭam uṣṇaṃ ca gāḍha-viṭ-pratipīḍitāḥ ।
sravanti sahasā raktaṃ tasya cāti-pravṛttitaḥ ।।

bhekābhaḥ pīḍyate duḥkhaiḥ śoṇita-kṣaya-saṃbhavaiḥ ।
hīna-varṇa-balotsāho hataujaḥ kaluṣendriyaḥ ।।

mudga-kodrava-jūrṇāhva-karīra-caṇakādibhiḥ ।
rūkṣaiḥ saṃgrāhibhir vāyuḥ sve sthāne kupito balī ।।

va-sthāne kupito balī
adho-vahāni srotāṃsi saṃrudhyādhaḥ praśoṣayan ।
purīṣaṃ vāta-viṇ-mūtra-saṅgaṃ kurvīta dāruṇam ।।

tena tīvrā rujā koṣṭha-pṛṣṭha-hṛt-pārśva-gā bhavet ।
ādhmānam udarāveṣṭo hṛl-lāso parikartanam ।।

vastau ca su-tarāṃ śūlaṃ gaṇḍa-śvayathu-saṃbhavaḥ ।
pavanasyordhva-gāmi-tvaṃ tataś chardy-a-ruci-jvarāḥ ।।

hṛd-roga-grahaṇī-doṣa-mūtra-saṅga-pravāhikāḥ ।
bādhirya-timira-śvāsa-śiro-ruk-kāsa-pīnasāḥ ।।

mano-vikāras tṛṣṇāsra-pitta-gulmodarādayaḥ ।
te te ca vāta-jā rogā jāyante bhṛśa-dāruṇāḥ ।।

dur-nāmnām ity udāvartaḥ paramo ayam upadravaḥ ।
vātābhibhūta-koṣṭhānāṃ tair vināpi sa jāyate ।।

saha-jāni tri-doṣāṇi yāni cābhyantare valau ।
sthitāni tāny a-sādhyāni yāpyante agni-balādibhiḥ ।।

dvandva-jāni dvitīyāyāṃ valau yāny āśritāni ca ।
kṛcchra-sādhyāni tāny āhuḥ pari-saṃvatsarāṇi ca ।।

bāhyāyāṃ tu valau jātāny eka-doṣolbaṇāni ca ।
arśāṃsi sukha-sādhyāni na cotpatitāni ca ।।

meḍhrādiṣv api vakṣyante yathā-svaṃ nābhi-jāni tu ।
gaṇḍū-padāsya-rūpāṇi picchilāni mṛdūni ca ।।

vyāno gṛhītvā śleṣmāṇaṃ karoty arśas tvaco bahiḥ ।
kīlopamaṃ sthira-kharaṃ carma-kīlaṃ tu taṃ viduḥ ।।

vātena todaḥ pāruṣyaṃ pittād asita-rakta-tā ।
śleṣmaṇā snigdha-tā tasya grathita-tvaṃ sa-varṇa-tā ।।

arśasāṃ praśame yatnam āśu kurvīta buddhi-mān ।
tāny āśu hi gudaṃ baddhvā kuryur baddha-gudodaram ।।

nidānasthāna
doṣair vyastaiḥ samastaiś ca bhayāc chokāc ca ṣaḍ-vidhaḥ ।
atīsāraḥ sa su-tarāṃ jāyate aty-ambu-pānataḥ ।।

kṛśa-śuṣkāmiṣā-sātmya-tila-piṣṭa-virūḍhakaiḥ ।
madya-rūkṣāti-mātrānnair arśobhiḥ sneha-vibhramāt ।।

kṛmibhyo vega-rodhāc ca tad-vidhaiḥ kupito anilaḥ ।
visraṃsayaty adho ab-dhātuṃ hatvā tenaiva cānalam ।।

vyāpadyānu-śakṛt koṣṭhaṃ purīṣaṃ drava-tāṃ nayan ।
prakalpate atisārāya lakṣaṇaṃ tasya bhāvinaḥ ।।

todo hṛd-guda-koṣṭheṣu gātra-sādo mala-grahaḥ ।
ādhmānam a-vipākaś ca tatra vātena viḍ-jalam ।।

alpālpaṃ śabda-śūlāḍhyaṃ vibaddham upaveśyate ।
rūkṣaṃ sa-phenam acchaṃ ca grathitaṃ vā muhur muhuḥ ।।

tathā dagdha-guḍābhāsaṃ sa-picchā-parikartikam ।
śuṣkāsyo bhraṣṭa-pāyuś ca hṛṣṭa-romā viniṣṭanan ।।

ṛṣṭa-romā vinaṣṭa-vāk
pittena pītam asitaṃ hāridraṃ śādvala-prabham ।
sa-raktam ati-dur-gandhaṃ -tṛṇ-mūrchā-sveda-dāha-vān ।।

-tṛṇ-mūrchā-sveda-dāha-vat
sa-śūlaṃ pāyu-saṃtāpa-pāka-vāñ chleṣmaṇā ghanam ।
picchilaṃ tantu-mac chvetaṃ snigdham āmaṃ kaphānvitam ।।

-pāka-vac chleṣmaṇā ghanam
abhīkṣṇam guru dur-gandhaṃ vibaddham anubaddha-ruk ।
nidrālur alaso anna-dviḍ alpālpaṃ sa-pravāhikam ।।

sa-roma-harṣaṃ sotkleśo guru-vasti-gudodaraḥ ।
kṛte apy a-kṛta-saṃjñaś ca sarvātmā sarva-lakṣaṇaḥ ।।

uru-vastir gurūdaraḥ
bhayena kṣobhite citte sa-pitto drāvayec chakṛt ।
vāyus tato atisāryeta kṣipram uṣṇaṃ dravaṃ plavam ।।

vāta-pitta-samaṃ liṅgair āhus tad-vac ca śokataḥ ।
atīsāraḥ samāsena dvi-dhā sāmo nir-āmakaḥ ।।

ve-dhā sāmo nir-āmakaḥ
sāsṛṅ nir-asras tatrādye gauravād apsu majjati ।
śakṛd dur-gandham āṭopa-viṣṭambhārti-prasekinaḥ ।।

viparīto nir-āmas tu kaphāt pakvo api majjati ।
atīsāreṣu yo nāti-yatna-vān grahaṇī-gadaḥ ।।

tasya syād agni-vidhvaṃsa-karair anyasya sevitaiḥ ।
sāmaṃ śakṛn nir-āmaṃ vā jīrṇe yenātisāryate ।।

so atīsāro ati-saraṇād āśu-kārī sva-bhāvataḥ ।
sāmaṃ sānnam a-jīrṇe anne jīrṇe pakvaṃ tu naiva vā ।।

a-kasmād vā muhur baddham a-kasmāc chithilaṃ muhuḥ ।
cira-kṛd grahaṇī-doṣaḥ saṃcayāc copaveśayet ।।

sa catur-dhā pṛthag doṣaiḥ saṃnipātāc ca jāyate ।
prāg-rūpaṃ tasya sadanaṃ cirāt pacanam amlakaḥ ।।

praseko vaktra-vairasyam a-rucis tṛṭ klamo bhramaḥ ।
ānaddhodara-tā chardiḥ karṇa-kṣveḍo antra-kūjanam ।।

sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kārśyaṃ dhūmakas tamako jvaraḥ ।
mūrchā śiro-rug viṣṭambhaḥ śvayathuḥ kara-pādayoḥ ।।

tatrānilāt tālu-śoṣas timiraṃ karṇayoḥ svanaḥ ।
pārśvoru-vaṅkṣaṇa-grīvā-rujābhīkṣṇaṃ viṣūcikā ।।

raseṣu gṛddhiḥ sarveṣu kṣut tṛṣṇā parikartikā ।
jīrṇe jīryati cādhmānaṃ bhukte svāsthyaṃ samaśnute ।।

vāta-hṛd-roga-gulmārśaḥ-plīha-pāṇḍu-tva-śaṅkitaḥ ।
cirād duḥkhaṃ dravaṃ śuṣkaṃ tanv āmaṃ śabda-phena-vat ।।

punaḥ punaḥ sṛjed varcaḥ pāyu-ruk-śvāsa-kāsa-vān ।
pittena nīla-pītābhaṃ pītābhaḥ sṛjati dravam ।।

ittena nīlaṃ pītābhaṃ ittena pīta-nīlābhaṃ
pūty-amlodgāra-hṛt-kaṇṭha-dāhā-ruci-tṛḍ-arditaḥ ।
śleṣmaṇā pacyate duḥkham annaṃ chardir a-rocakaḥ ।।

āsyopadeha-niṣṭhīva-kāsa-hṛl-lāsa-pīnasāḥ ।
hṛdayaṃ manyate styānam udaraṃ stimitaṃ guru ।।

āsyopadeha-mādhurya- -kāsa-ṣṭhīvana-pīnasāḥ
udgāro duṣṭa-madhuraḥ sadanaṃ strīṣv a-harṣaṇam ।
bhinnāma-śleṣma-saṃsṛṣṭa-guru-varcaḥ-pravartanam ।।

a-kṛśasyāpi daurbalyaṃ sarva-je sarva-saṃkaraḥ ।
vibhāge aṅgasya ye coktā viṣamādyās trayo agnayaḥ ।।
te api syur grahaṇī-doṣāḥ samas tu svāsthya-kāraṇam ।।vāta-vyādhy-aśmarī-kuṣṭha-mehodara-bhagandarāḥ ।।arśāṃsi grahaṇīty aṣṭau mahā-rogāḥ su-dus-tarāḥ ।।
nidānasthāna
vasti-vasti-śiro-meḍhra-kaṭī-vṛṣaṇa-pāyavaḥ ।
eka-saṃbandhanāḥ proktā gudāsthi-vivarāśrayāḥ ।।

adho-mukho api vastir hi mūtra-vāhi-sirā-mukhaiḥ ।
pārśvebhyaḥ pūryate sūkṣmaiḥ syandamānair an-āratam ।।

yais tair eva praviśyainaṃ doṣāḥ kurvanti viṃśatim ।
mūtrāghātān pramehāṃś ca kṛcchrān marma-samāśrayān ।।

vasti-vaṅkṣaṇa-meḍhrārti-yukto alpālpaṃ muhur muhuḥ ।
mūtrayed vāta-je kṛcchre paitte pītaṃ sa-dāha-ruk ।।

raktaṃ vā kapha-je vasti-meḍhra-gaurava-śopha-vān ।
sa-picchaṃ sa-vibandhaṃ ca sarvaiḥ sarvātmakaṃ malaiḥ ।।

yadā vāyur mukhaṃ vaster āvṛtya pariśoṣayet ।
mūtraṃ sa-pittaṃ sa-kaphaṃ sa-śukraṃ vā tadā kramāt ।।

saṃjāyate aśmarī ghorā pittād gor iva rocanā ।
śleṣmāśrayā ca sarvā syād athāsyāḥ pūrva-lakṣaṇam ।।

vasty-ādhmānaṃ tad-āsanna-deśeṣu parito ati-ruk ।
mūtre ca basta-gandha-tvaṃ mūtra-kṛcchraṃ jvaro a-ruciḥ ।।

ūtre basta-sa-gandha-tvaṃ
sāmānya-liṅgaṃ ruṅ nābhi-sevanī-vasti-mūrdhasu ।
viśīrṇa-dhāraṃ mūtraṃ syāt tayā mārga-nirodhane ।।

athā mārga-nirodhane
tad-vyapāyāt sukhaṃ mehed acchaṃ gomedakopamam ।
tat-saṃkṣobhāt kṣate sāsram āyāsāc cāti-rug bhavet ।।

tatra vātād bhṛśārty-ārto dantān khādati vepate ।
mṛdnāti mehanaṃ nābhiṃ pīḍayaty a-niśaṃ kvaṇan ।।

sānilaṃ muñcati śakṛn muhur mehati bindu-śaḥ ।
śyāvā rūkṣāśmarī cāsya syāc citā kaṇṭakair iva ।।

pittena dahyate vastiḥ pacyamāna ivoṣma-vān ।
bhallātakāsthi-saṃsthānā raktā pītāsitāśmarī ।।

akta-pītāsitāśmarī
vastir nistudyata iva śleṣmaṇā śītalo guruḥ ।
aśmarī mahatī ślakṣṇā madhu-varṇātha-vā sitā ।।

etā bhavanti bālānāṃ teṣām eva ca bhūyasā ।
āśrayopacayālpa-tvād grahaṇāharaṇe sukhāḥ ।।

śukrāśmarī tu mahatāṃ jāyate śukra-dhāraṇāt ।
sthānāc cyutam a-muktaṃ hi muṣkayor antare anilaḥ ।।

śoṣayaty upasaṃgṛhya śukraṃ tac chuṣkam aśmarī ।
vasti-ruk-kṛcchra-mūtra-tva-muṣka-śvayathu-kāriṇī ।।

tasyām utpanna-mātrāyāṃ śukram eti vilīyate ।
pīḍite tv avakāśe asminn aśmary eva ca śarkarā ।।

aṇu-śo vāyunā bhinnā sā tv asminn anuloma-ge ।
nireti saha mūtreṇa pratilome vibadhyate ।।

mūtra-saṃdhāriṇaḥ kuryād ruddhvā vaster mukhaṃ marut ।
mūtra-saṅgaṃ rujaṃ kaṇḍūṃ kadā-cic ca sva-dhāmataḥ ।।

pracyāvya vastim udvṛttaṃ garbhābhaṃ sthūla-viplutam ।
karoti tatra rug-dāha-spandanodveṣṭanāni ca ।।

bindu-śaś ca pravarteta mūtraṃ vastau tu pīḍite ।
dhārayā dvi-vidho apy eṣa vāta-vastir iti smṛtaḥ ।।

dus-taro dus-tara-taro dvitīyaḥ prabalānilaḥ ।
śakṛn-mārgasya vasteś ca vāyur antaram āśritaḥ ।।

aṣṭhīlābhaṃ ghanaṃ granthiṃ karoty a-calam unnatam ।
vātāṣṭhīleti sādhmāna-viṇ-mūtrānila-saṅga-kṛt ।।

vi-guṇaḥ kuṇḍalī-bhūto vastau tīvra-vyatho anilaḥ ।
āvidhya mūtraṃ bhramati sa-stambhodveṣṭa-gauravaḥ ।।

āviśya mūtraṃ bhramati
mūtram alpālpam atha-vā vimuñcati śakṛt sṛjan ।
vāta-kuṇḍalikety eṣā mūtraṃ tu vidhṛtaṃ ciram ।।

na nireti vibaddhaṃ vā mūtrātītaṃ tad alpa-ruk ।
vidhāraṇāt pratihataṃ vātodāvartitaṃ yadā ।।

nābher adhas-tād udaraṃ mūtram āpūrayet tadā ।
kuryāt tīvra-rug ādhmānam a-paktiṃ mala-saṃgraham ।।

tan mūtra-jaṭharaṃ chidra-vaiguṇyenānilena vā ।
ākṣiptam alpaṃ mūtraṃ tad vastau nāle atha-vā maṇau ।।

ākṣiptam alpaṃ mūtrasya
sthitvā sravec chanaiḥ paścāt sa-rujaṃ vātha nī-rujam ।
mūtrotsaṅgaḥ sa vicchinna-tac-cheṣa-guru-śephasaḥ ।।

a-rujaṃ vātha-vā-rujam ūtrotsaṅgaḥ sa vicchinnas ūtrotsaṅgaḥ sa vicchinnaṃ 
ac-cheṣa-guru-śephasaḥ
antar vasti-mukhe vṛttaḥ sthiro alpaḥ sahasā bhavet ।
aśmarī-tulya-rug granthir mūtra-granthiḥ sa ucyate ।।

mūtritasya striyaṃ yāto vāyunā śukram uddhatam ।
sthānāc cyutaṃ mūtrayataḥ prāk paścād vā pravartate ।।

bhasmodaka-pratīkāśaṃ mūtra-śukraṃ tad ucyate ।
rūkṣa-dur-balayor vātād udāvartaṃ śakṛd yadā ।।

dāvṛttaṃ śakṛd yadā
mūtra-sroto anuparyeti saṃsṛṣṭaṃ śakṛtā tadā ।
mūtraṃ viṭ-tulya-gandhaṃ syād viḍ-vighātaṃ tam ādiśet ।।

pittaṃ vyāyāma-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-bhojanādhvātapādibhiḥ ।
pravṛddhaṃ vāyunā kṣiptaṃ vasty-upasthārti-dāha-vat ।।

mūtraṃ pravartayet pītaṃ sa-raktaṃ raktam eva vā ।
uṣṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ kṛcchrād uṣṇa-vātaṃ vadanti tam ।।

rūkṣasya klānta-dehasya vasti-sthau pitta-mārutau ।
mūtra-kṣayaṃ sa-rug-dāhaṃ janayetāṃ tad-āhvayam ।।

pittaṃ kapho dvāv api vā saṃhanyete anilena cet ।
kṛcchrān mūtraṃ tadā pītaṃ raktaṃ śvetaṃ ghanaṃ sṛjet ।।

sa-dāhaṃ rocanā-śaṅkha-cūrṇa-varṇaṃ bhavec ca tat ।
śuṣkaṃ samasta-varṇaṃ vā mūtra-sādaṃ vadanti tam ।।

iti vistarataḥ proktā rogā mūtrā-pravṛtti-jāḥ ।
nidāna-lakṣaṇair ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyante ati-pravṛtti-jāḥ ।।

nidānasthāna
pramehā viṃśatis tatra śleṣmato daśa pittataḥ ।
ṣaṭ catvāro anilāt teṣāṃ medo-mūtra-kaphāvaham ।।

anna-pāna-kriyā-jātaṃ yat prāyas tat pravartakam ।
svādv-amla-lavaṇa-snigdha-guru-picchila-śītalam ।।

nava-dhānya-surānūpa-māṃsekṣu-guḍa-go-rasam ।
eka-sthānāsana-ratiḥ śayanaṃ vidhi-varjitam ।।

vastim āśritya kurute pramehān dūṣitaḥ kaphaḥ ।
dūṣayitvā vapuḥ-kleda-sveda-medo-rasāmiṣam ।।

-sveda-medo-vasāmiṣam
pittaṃ raktam api kṣīṇe kaphādau mūtra-saṃśrayam ।
dhātūn vastim upānīya tat-kṣaye api ca mārutaḥ ।।

sādhya-yāpya-parityājyā mehās tenaiva tad-bhavāḥ ।
samāsam a-kriya-tayā mahātyaya-tayāpi ca ।।

sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ teṣāṃ prabhūtāvila-mūtra-tā ।
doṣa-dūṣyā-viśeṣe api tat-saṃyoga-viśeṣataḥ ।।

rabhūtākula-mūtra-tā
mūtra-varṇādi-bhedena bhedo meheṣu kalpyate ।
acchaṃ bahu sitaṃ śītaṃ nir-gandham udakopamam ।।

mehaty udaka-mehena kiñ-cic cāvila-picchilam ।
ikṣo rasam ivāty-arthaṃ madhuraṃ cekṣu-mehataḥ ।।

sāndrī-bhavet paryuṣitaṃ sāndra-mehena mehati ।
surā-mehī surā-tulyam upary accham adho ghanam ।।

saṃhṛṣṭa-romā piṣṭena piṣṭa-vad bahalaṃ sitam ।
śukrābhaṃ śukra-miśraṃ vā śukra-mehī pramehati ।।

iṣṭa-vad bahulaṃ sitam
mūrtāṇūn sikatā-mehī sikatā-rūpiṇo malān ।
śīta-mehī su-bahu-śo madhuraṃ bhṛśa-śītalam ।।

ūtrāṇūn sikatā-mehī ūtre aṇūn sikatā-mehī
śanaiḥ śanaiḥ śanair-mehī mandaṃ mandaṃ pramehati ।
lālā-tantu-yutaṃ mūtraṃ lālā-mehena picchilam ।।

gandha-varṇa-rasa-sparśaiḥ kṣāreṇa kṣāra-toya-vat ।
nīla-mehena nīlābhaṃ kāla-mehī maṣī-nibham ।।

hāridra-mehī kaṭukaṃ haridrā-saṃnibhaṃ dahat ।
visraṃ māñjiṣṭha-mehena mañjiṣṭhā-salilopamam ।।

visram uṣṇaṃ sa-lavaṇaṃ raktābhaṃ rakta-mehataḥ ।
vasā-mehī vasā-miśraṃ vasāṃ vā mūtrayen muhuḥ ।।

majjānaṃ majja-miśraṃ vā majja-mehī muhur muhuḥ ।
hastī matta ivājasraṃ mūtraṃ vega-vivarjitam ।।

ajjābhaṃ majja-miśraṃ vā
sa-lasīkaṃ vibaddhaṃ ca hasti-mehī pramehati ।
madhu-mehī madhu-samaṃ jāyate sa kila dvi-dhā ।।

adhu-mehe madhu-samaṃ
kruddhe dhātu-kṣayād vāyau doṣāvṛta-pathe atha-vā ।
āvṛto doṣa-liṅgāni so a-nimittaṃ pradarśayet ।।

oṣāvṛta-pathe api vā
kṣīṇaḥ kṣaṇāt kṣaṇāt pūrṇo bhajate kṛcchra-sādhya-tām ।
kālenopekṣitāḥ sarve yad yānti madhu-meha-tām ।।

madhuraṃ yac ca sarveṣu prāyo madhv iva mehati ।
sarve api madhu-mehākhyā mādhuryāc ca tanor ataḥ ।।

a-vipāko a-ruciś chardir nidrā kāsaḥ sa-pīnasaḥ ।
upadravāḥ prajāyante mehānāṃ kapha-janmanām ।।

vasti-mehanayos todo muṣkāvadaraṇaṃ jvaraḥ ।
dāhas tṛṣṇāmlako mūrchā viḍ-bhedaḥ pitta-janmanām ।।

vātikānām udāvarta-kampa-hṛd-graha-lola-tāḥ ।
śūlam unnidra-tā śoṣaḥ kāsaḥ śvāsaś ca jāyate ।।

-kaṇṭha-hṛd-graha-lola-tāḥ
śarāvikā kacchapikā jālinī vinatālajī ।
masūrikā sarṣapikā putriṇī sa-vidārikā ।।

utriṇī ca vidārikā
vidradhiś ceti piṭikāḥ pramehopekṣayā daśa ।
saṃdhi-marmasu jāyante māṃsaleṣu ca dhāmasu ।।

antonnatā madhya-nimnā śyāvā kleda-rujānvitā ।
śarāva-māna-saṃsthānā piṭikā syāc charāvikā ।।

avagāḍhārti-nistodā mahā-vastu-parigrahā ।
ślakṣṇā kacchapa-pṛṣṭhābhā piṭikā kacchapī matā ।।

stabdhā sirā-jāla-vatī snigdha-srāvā mahāśayā ।
rujā-nistoda-bahulā sūkṣma-cchidrā ca jālinī ।।

nigdha-srāvā mahāśrayā
avagāḍha-rujā-kledā pṛṣṭhe vā jaṭhare api vā ।
mahatī piṭikā nīlā vinatā vinatā smṛtā ।।

dahati tvacam utthāne bhṛśaṃ kaṣṭā visarpiṇī ।
rakta-kṛṣṇāti-tṛṭ-sphoṭa-dāha-moha-jvarālajī ।।

māna-saṃsthānayos tulyā masūreṇa masūrikā ।
sarṣapā-māna-saṃsthānā kṣipra-pākā mahā-rujā ।।

sarṣapī sarṣapā-tulya-piṭikā-parivāritā ।
putriṇī mahatī bhūri-su-sūkṣma-piṭikācitā ।।

arṣapā sarṣapā-tulya- -su-sūkṣma-piṭikāvṛtā 
-su-sūkṣma-piṭikānvitā
vidārī-kanda-vad vṛttā kaṭhinā ca vidārikā ।
vidradhir vakṣyate anya-tra tatrādyaṃ piṭikā-trayam ।।

putriṇī ca vidārī ca duḥ-sahā bahu-medasaḥ ।
sahyāḥ pittolbaṇās tv anyāḥ saṃbhavanty alpa-medasaḥ ।।
tāsu meha-vaśāc ca syād doṣodreko yathā-yatham ।।prameheṇa vināpy etā jāyante duṣṭa-medasaḥ ।।tāvac ca nopalakṣyante yāvad vastu-parigrahaḥ ।।
hāridra-varṇaṃ raktaṃ vā meha-prāg-rūpa-varjitam ।
yo mūtrayen na taṃ mehaṃ rakta-pittaṃ tu tad viduḥ ।।

akta-pittaṃ tu taṃ viduḥ akta-pittaṃ ca tad viduḥ
svedo aṅga-gandhaḥ śithila-tvam aṅge śayyāsana-svapna-sukhābhiṣaṅgaḥ ।
hṛn-netra-jihvā-śravaṇopadeho ghanāṅga-tā keśa-nakhāti-vṛddhiḥ ।।

śayyāsana-sthāna-sukhābhilāṣaḥ
śīta-priya-tvaṃ gala-tālu-śoṣo mādhuryam āsye kara-pāda-dāhaḥ ।
bhaviṣyato meha-gaṇasya rūpaṃ mūtre abhidhāvanti pipīlikāś ca ।।

dṛṣṭvā pramehaṃ madhuraṃ sa-picchaṃ madhūpamaṃ syād vividho vicāraḥ ।
saṃpūraṇād vā kapha-saṃbhavaḥ syāt kṣīṇeṣu doṣeṣv anilātmako vā ।।

aṃtarpaṇād vā kapha-saṃbhavaḥ syāt
sa-pūrva-rūpāḥ kapha-pitta-mehāḥ krameṇa ye vāta-kṛtāś ca mehāḥ ।
sādhyā na te pitta-kṛtās tu yāpyāḥ sādhyās tu medo yadi nāti-duṣṭam ।।

ādhyāś ca medo yadi nāti-duṣṭam

nidānasthāna
bhuktaiḥ paryuṣitāty-uṣṇa-rūkṣa-śuṣka-vidāhibhiḥ ।
jihma-śayyā-viceṣṭābhis tais taiś cāsṛk-pradūṣaṇaiḥ ।।

duṣṭa-tvaṅ-māṃsa-medo-'sthi-snāyv-asṛk-kaṇḍarāśrayaḥ ।
yaḥ śopho bahir antar vā mahā-mūlo mahā-rujaḥ ।।

uṣṭas tvaṅ-māṃsa-medo-'sthi-
vṛttaḥ syād āyato yo vā smṛtaḥ ṣo-ḍhā sa vidradhiḥ ।
doṣaiḥ pṛthak samuditaiḥ śoṇitena kṣatena ca ।।

bāhyo atra tatra tatrāṅge dāruṇo grathitonnataḥ ।
āntaro dāruṇa-taro gambhīro gulma-vad ghanaḥ ।।

valmīka-vat samucchrāyī śīghra-ghāty agni-śastra-vat ।
nābhi-vasti-yakṛt-plīha-kloma-hṛt-kukṣi-vaṅkṣaṇe ।।

syād vṛkkayor apāne ca vātāt tatrāti-tīvra-ruk ।
śyāvāruṇaś cirotthāna-pāko viṣama-saṃsthitiḥ ।।

yād vṛkkayor apāne vā
vyadha-ccheda-bhramānāha-spanda-sarpaṇa-śabda-vān ।
rakta-tāmrāsitaḥ pittāt tṛṇ-moha-jvara-dāha-vān ।।

kṣiprotthāna-prapākaś ca pāṇḍuḥ kaṇḍū-yutaḥ kaphāt ।
sotkleśa-śītaka-stambha-jṛmbhā-rocaka-gauravaḥ ।।

cirotthāna-vipākaś ca saṃkīrṇaḥ saṃnipātataḥ ।
sāmarthyāc cātra vibhajed bāhyābhyantara-lakṣaṇam ।।

irotthāna-prapākaś ca
kṛṣṇa-sphoṭāvṛtaḥ śyāvas tīvra-dāha-rujā-jvaraḥ ।
pitta-liṅgo asṛjā bāhyaḥ strīṇām eva tathāntaraḥ ।।

śastrādyair abhighātena kṣate vā-pathya-kāriṇaḥ ।
kṣatoṣmā vāyu-vikṣiptaḥ sa-raktaṃ pittam īrayan ।।

a-raktaṃ pittam īrayet
pittāsṛg-lakṣaṇaṃ kuryād vidradhiṃ bhūry-upadravam ।
teṣūpadrava-bhedaś ca smṛto adhiṣṭhāna-bhedataḥ ।।

nābhyāṃ hidhmā bhaved vastau mūtraṃ kṛcchreṇa pūti ca ।
śvāso yakṛti rodhas tu plīhny ucchvāsasya tṛṭ punaḥ ।।

gala-grahaś ca klomni syāt sarvāṅga-pragraho hṛdi ।
pramohas tamakaḥ kāso hṛdaye ghaṭṭanaṃ vyathā ।।

kukṣi-pārśvāntarāṃsārtiḥ kukṣāv āṭopa-janma ca ।
sakthnor graho vaṅkṣaṇayor vṛkkayoḥ kaṭi-pṛṣṭhayoḥ ।।

pārśvayoś ca vyathā pāyau pavanasya nirodhanam ।
āma-pakva-vidagdha-tvaṃ teṣāṃ śopha-vad ādiśet ।।

nābher ūrdhvaṃ mukhāt pakvāḥ prasravanty adhare gudāt ।
gudāsyān nābhi-jo vidyād doṣaṃ kledāc ca vidradhau ।।

bhābhyāṃ nābhi-jo vidyād
yathā-svaṃ vraṇa-vat tatra vivarjyaḥ saṃnipāta-jaḥ ।
pakvo hṛn-nābhi-vasti-stho bhinno antar bahir eva vā ।।

pakvaś cāntaḥ sravan vaktrāt kṣīṇasyopadravānvitaḥ ।
evam eva stana-sirā vivṛtāḥ prāpya yoṣitām ।।

sūtānāṃ garbhiṇīnāṃ vā saṃbhavec chvayathur ghanaḥ ।
stane sa-dugdhe a-dugdhe vā bāhya-vidradhi-lakṣaṇaḥ ।।

nāḍīnāṃ sūkṣma-vaktra-tvāt kanyānāṃ na sa jāyate ।
kruddho ruddha-gatir vāyuḥ śopha-śūla-karaś caran ।।

anyānāṃ tu na jāyate ruddho an-ūrdhva-gatir vāyuḥ
muṣkau vaṅkṣaṇataḥ prāpya phala-kośābhivāhinīḥ ।
prapīḍya dhamanīr vṛddhiṃ karoti phala-kośayoḥ ।।

doṣāsra-medo-mūtrāntraiḥ sa vṛddhiḥ sapta-dhā gadaḥ ।
mūtrāntra-jāv apy anilād dhetu-bhedas tu kevalam ।।

vāta-pūrṇa-dṛti-sparśo rūkṣo vātād a-hetu-ruk ।
pakvodumbara-saṃkāśaḥ pittād dāhoṣma-pāka-vān ।।

kaphāc chīto guruḥ snigdhaḥ kaṇḍū-mān kaṭhino alpa-ruk ।
kṛṣṇa-sphoṭāvṛtaḥ pitta-vṛddhi-liṅgaś ca raktataḥ ।।

ṛṣṇaḥ sphoṭāvṛtaḥ pitta-
kapha-van medasā vṛddhir mṛdus tāla-phalopamaḥ ।
mūtra-dhāraṇa-śīlasya mūtra-jaḥ sa tu gacchataḥ ।।

ambhobhiḥ pūrṇa-dṛti-vat kṣobhaṃ yāti sa-ruṅ mṛduḥ ।
mūtra-kṛcchram adhas-tāc ca valayaṃ phala-kośayoḥ ।।

vāta-kopibhir āhāraiḥ śīta-toyāvagāhanaiḥ ।
dhāraṇeraṇa-bhārādhva-viṣamāṅga-pravartanaiḥ ।।

kṣobhaṇaiḥ kṣubhito anyaiś ca kṣudrāntrāvayavaṃ yadā ।
pavano vi-guṇī-kṛtya sva-niveśād adho nayet ।।

avano dvi-guṇī-kṛtya kuryād vaṅkṣaṇa-saṃdhi-stho granthy-ābhaṃ śvayathuṃ tadā ।।
upekṣyamāṇasya ca muṣka-vṛddhim ādhmāna-ruk-stambha-vatīṃ sa vāyuḥ ।।prapīḍito antaḥ svana-vān prayāti pradhmāpayann eti punaś ca muktaḥ ।।antra-vṛddhir a-sādhyo ayaṃ vāta-vṛddhi-samākṛtiḥ ।।iti vṛddhi-nidānam atha gulma-nidānam ।।
rūkṣa-kṛṣṇāruṇa-sirā-tantu-jāla-gavākṣitaḥ ।
gulmo aṣṭa-dhā pṛthag doṣaiḥ saṃsṛṣṭair nicayaṃ gataiḥ ।।

ārtavasya ca doṣeṇa nārīṇāṃ jāyate aṣṭamaḥ ।
jvara-cchardy-atisārādyair vamanādyaiś ca karmabhiḥ ।।

karśito vātalāny atti śītaṃ vāmbu bubhukṣitaḥ ।
yaḥ pibaty anu cānnāni laṅghana-plavanādikam ।।

śītaṃ cāmbu bubhukṣitaḥ
sevate deha-saṃkṣobhi cchardiṃ vā samudīrayet ।
an-udīrṇām udīrṇān vā vātādīn na vimuñcati ।।

sneha-svedāv an-abhyasya śodhanaṃ vā niṣevate ।
śuddho vāśu vidāhīni bhajate syandanāni vā ।।

vātolbaṇās tasya malāḥ pṛthak kruddhā dvi-śo atha-vā ।
sarve vā rakta-yuktā vā mahā-sroto-'nuśāyinaḥ ।।

ūrdhvādho-mārgam āvṛtya kurvate śūla-pūrvakam ।
sparśopalabhyaṃ gulmākhyam utplutaṃ granthi-rūpiṇam ।।

nnataṃ granthi-rūpiṇam
karśanāt kapha-viṭ-pittair mārgasyāvaraṇena vā ।
vāyuḥ kṛtāśrayaḥ koṣṭhe raukṣyāt kāṭhinyam āgataḥ ।।

sva-tantraḥ svāśraye duṣṭaḥ para-tantraḥ parāśraye ।
piṇḍita-tvād a-mūrto api mūrta-tvam iva saṃśritaḥ ।।

gulma ity ucyate vasti-nābhi-hṛt-pārśva-saṃśrayaḥ ।
vātān manyā-śiraḥ-śūlaṃ jvara-plīhāntra-kūjanam ।।

vyadhaḥ sūcyeva viṭ-saṅgaḥ kṛcchrād ucchvasanaṃ muhuḥ ।
stambho gātre mukhe śoṣaḥ kārśyaṃ viṣama-vahni-tā ।।

rūkṣa-kṛṣṇa-tvag-ādi-tvaṃ cala-tvād anilasya ca ।
a-nirūpita-saṃsthāna-sthāna-vṛddhi-kṣaya-vyathaḥ ।।

pipīlikā-vyāpta iva gulmaḥ sphurati tudyate ।
pittād dāho amlako mūrchā-viḍ-bheda-sveda-tṛḍ-jvarāḥ ।।

hāridra-tvaṃ tvag-ādyeṣu gulmaś ca sparśanā-sahaḥ ।
dūyate dīpyate soṣmā sva-sthānaṃ dahatīva ca ।।

kaphāt staimityam a-ruciḥ sadanaṃ śiśira-jvaraḥ ।
pīnasālasya-hṛl-lāsa-kāsa-śukla-tvag-ādi-tāḥ ।।

gulmo avagāḍhaḥ kaṭhino guruḥ suptaḥ sthiro alpa-ruk ।
sva-doṣa-sthāna-dhāmānaḥ sve sve kāle ca ruk-karāḥ ।।

prāyas trayas tu dvandvotthā gulmāḥ saṃsṛṣṭa-lakṣaṇāḥ ।
sarva-jas tīvra-rug-dāhaḥ śīghra-pākī ghanonnataḥ ।।

so a-sādhyo rakta-gulmas tu striyā eva prajāyate ।
ṛtau vā nava-sūtā vā yadi vā yoni-rogiṇī ।।

sevate vātalāni strī kruddhas tasyāḥ samīraṇaḥ ।
niruṇaddhy ārtavaṃ yonyāṃ prati-māsam avasthitam ।।

kukṣiṃ karoti tad-garbha-liṅgam āviṣ-karoti ca ।
hṛl-lāsa-daurhṛda-stanya-darśana-kṣāma-tādikam ।।

krameṇa vāyu-saṃsargāt pitta-yoni-tayā ca tat ।
śoṇitaṃ kurute tasyā vāta-pittottha-gulma-jān ।।

ruk-stambha-dāhātīsāra-tṛḍ-jvarādīn upadravān ।
garbhāśaye ca su-tarāṃ śūlaṃ duṣṭāsṛg-āśraye ।।

yonyāś ca srāva-daurgandhya-toda-spandana-vedanāḥ ।
na cāṅgair garbha-vad gulmaḥ sphuraty api tu śūla-vān ।।

-toda-sphuraṇa-vedanāḥ -kleda-svedana-vedanāḥ
piṇḍī-bhūtaḥ sa evāsyāḥ kadā-cit spandate cirāt ।
na cāsyā vardhate kukṣir gulma eva tu vardhate ।।

sva-doṣa-saṃśrayo gulmaḥ sarvo bhavati tena saḥ ।
pākaṃ cireṇa bhajate naiva vā vidradhiḥ punaḥ ।।

pacyate śīghram aty-arthaṃ duṣṭa-raktāśraya-tvataḥ ।
ataḥ śīghra-vidāhi-tvād vidradhiḥ so abhidhīyate ।।

gulme antar-āśraye vasti-kukṣi-hṛt-plīha-vedanāḥ ।
agni-varṇa-bala-bhraṃśo vegānāṃ cā-pravartanam ।।

-kukṣi-hṛt-pārśva-vedanāḥ
ato viparyayo bāhye koṣṭhāṅgeṣu tu nāti-ruk ।
vaivarṇyam avakāśasya bahir unnata-tādhikam ।।

sāṭopam aty-ugra-rujam ādhmānam udare bhṛśam ।
ūrdhvādho-vāta-rodhena tam ānāhaṃ pracakṣate ।।

ghano aṣṭhīlopamo granthir aṣṭhīlordhvaṃ samunnataḥ ।
ānāha-liṅgas tiryak tu pratyaṣṭhīlā tad-ākṛtiḥ ।।

ānāha-liṅgas tiryak ca
pakvāśayād gudopasthaṃ vāyus tīvra-rujaḥ prayān ।
tūṇī pratūṇī tu bhavet sa evāto viparyaye ।।

udgāra-bāhulya-purīṣa-bandha-tṛpty-a-kṣama-tvāntra-vikūjanāni ।
āṭopam ādhmānam a-pakti-śaktim āsanna-gulmasya vadanti cihnam ।।

āṭopam ādhmānam a-pakty-a-śaktim

nidānasthāna
rogāḥ sarve api mande agnau su-tarām udarāṇi tu ।
a-jīrṇān malinaiś cānnair jāyante mala-saṃcayāt ।।

ūrdhvādho dhātavo ruddhvā vāhinīr ambu-vāhinīḥ ।
prāṇāgny-apānān saṃdūṣya kuryus tvaṅ-māṃsa-saṃdhi-gāḥ ।।

ādhmāpya kukṣim udaram aṣṭa-dhā tac ca bhidyate ।
pṛthag doṣaiḥ samastaiś ca plīha-baddha-kṣatodakaiḥ ।।

tenārtāḥ śuṣka-tālv-oṣṭhāḥ śūna-pāda-karodarāḥ ।
naṣṭa-ceṣṭā-balāhārāḥ kṛśāḥ pradhmāta-kukṣayaḥ ।।

syuḥ preta-rūpāḥ puruṣā bhāvinas tasya lakṣaṇam ।
kṣun-nāśo annaṃ cirāt sarvaṃ sa-vidāhaṃ ca pacyate ।।

a-vidāhaṃ vipacyate
jīrṇā-jīrṇaṃ na jānāti sauhityaṃ sahate na ca ।
kṣīyate balataḥ śaśvac chvasity alpe api ceṣṭite ।।

vṛddhir viṣo a-pravṛttiś ca kiñ-cic chophaś ca pādayoḥ ।
rug-vasti-saṃdhau tata-tā laghv-alpā-bhojanair api ।।

ṛddhir viṣo a-pravṛttir vā
rājī-janma valī-nāśo jaṭhare jaṭhareṣu tu ।
sarveṣu tandrā sadanaṃ mala-saṅgo alpa-vahni-tā ।।

dāhaḥ śvayathur ādhmānam ante salila-saṃbhavaḥ ।
sarvaṃ tv a-toyam aruṇam a-śophaṃ nāti-bhārikam ।।

gavākṣitaṃ sirā-jālaiḥ sadā guḍaguḍāyate ।
nābhim antraṃ ca viṣṭabhya vegaṃ kṛtvā praṇaśyati ।।

māruto hṛt-kaṭī-nābhi-pāyu-vaṅkṣaṇa-vedanāḥ ।
sa-śabdo niścared vāyur viḍ baddhā mūtram alpakam ।।

-pāyu-vaṅkṣaṇa-vedanā
nāti-mando analo laulyaṃ na ca syād vi-rasaṃ mukham ।
tatra vātodare śophaḥ pāṇi-pān-muṣka-kukṣiṣu ।।

kukṣi-pārśvodara-kaṭī-pṛṣṭha-ruk parva-bhedanam ।
śuṣka-kāso aṅga-mardo adho-guru-tā mala-saṃgrahaḥ ।।

śyāvāruṇa-tvag-ādi-tvam a-kasmād vṛddhi-hrāsa-vat ।
sa-toda-bhedam udaraṃ tanu-kṛṣṇa-sirā-tatam ।।

anu kṛṣṇa-sirā-tatam
ādhmāta-dṛti-vac chabdam āhataṃ prakaroti ca ।
vāyuś cātra sa-ruk-śabdo vicaret sarvato-gatiḥ ।।

pittodare jvaro mūrchā dāhas tṛṭ kaṭukāsya-tā ।
bhramo atīsāraḥ pīta-tvaṃ tvag-ādāv udaraṃ harit ।।

pīta-tāmra-sirānaddhaṃ sa-svedaṃ soṣma dahyate ।
dhūmāyati mṛdu-sparśaṃ kṣipra-pākaṃ pradūyate ।।

hūmāyate mṛdu-sparśaṃ
śleṣmodare aṅga-sadanaṃ svāpaḥ śvayathu-gauravam ।
nidrotkleśā-ruci-śvāsa-kāsa-śukla-tvag-ādi-tā ।।

vāpa-śvayathu-gauravam
udaraṃ stimitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ śukla-rājī-tataṃ mahat ।
cirābhivṛddhi kaṭhinaṃ śīta-sparśaṃ guru sthiram ।।

daraṃ stimitaṃ snigdhaṃ
tri-doṣa-kopanais tais taiḥ strī-dattaiś ca rajo-malaiḥ ।
gara-dūṣī-viṣādyaiś ca sa-raktāḥ saṃcitā malāḥ ।।

koṣṭhaṃ prāpya vikurvāṇāḥ śoṣa-mūrchā-bhramānvitam ।
kuryus tri-liṅgam udaraṃ śīghra-pākaṃ su-dāruṇam ।।

bādhate tac ca su-tarāṃ śīta-vātābhra-darśane ।
aty-āśitasya saṃkṣobhād yāna-yānādi-ceṣṭitaiḥ ।।

śīta-vātābhra-darśanaiḥ
ati-vyavāya-karmādhva-vamana-vyādhi-karśanaiḥ ।
vāma-pārśvāśritaḥ plīhā cyutaḥ sthānād vivardhate ।।

śoṇitaṃ vā rasādibhyo vivṛddhaṃ taṃ vivardhayet ।
so aṣṭhīlevāti-kaṭhinaḥ prāk tataḥ kūrma-pṛṣṭha-vat ।।

rākṛtaḥ kūrma-pṛṣṭha-vat
krameṇa vardhamānaś ca kukṣāv udaram āvahet ।
śvāsa-kāsa-pipāsāsya-vairasyādhmāna-rug-jvaraiḥ ।।

pāṇḍu-tva-mūrchā-chardībhir dāha-mohaiś ca saṃyutam ।
aruṇābhaṃ vi-varṇaṃ vā nīla-hāridra-rāji-mat ।।

āṇḍu-tva-mūrchāti-chardi- -dāha-mohaiś ca saṃyutam
udāvarta-rujānāhair moha-tṛḍ-dahana-jvaraiḥ ।
gauravā-ruci-kāṭhinyair vidyāt tatra malān kramāt ।।

dāvarta-rug-ānāhair
plīha-vad dakṣiṇāt pārśvāt kuryād yakṛd api cyutam ।
pakṣma-vālaiḥ sahānnena bhuktair baddhāyane gude ।।

dur-nāmabhir udāvartair anyair vāntropalepibhiḥ ।
varcaḥ-pitta-kaphān ruddhvā karoti kupito anilaḥ ।।

nnair vāntropalepibhiḥ
apāno jaṭharaṃ tena syur dāha-jvara-tṛṭ-kṣavāḥ ।
kāsa-śvāsoru-sadanaṃ śiro-hṛn-nābhi-pāyu-ruk ।।

yur dāha-jvara-tṛṭ-kṣudhāḥ yur dāha-jvara-tṛṭ-kṣutaḥ
mala-saṅgo a-ruciś chardir udaraṃ mūḍha-mārutam ।
sthiraṃ nīlāruṇa-sirā-rājī-naddham a-rāji vā ।।

nābher upari ca prāyo go-pucchākṛti jāyate ।
asthy-ādi-śalyaiḥ sānnaiś ced bhuktair aty-aśanena vā ।।

sthy-ādi-śalyaiḥ sānnaiś ca
bhidyate pacyate vāntraṃ tac-chidraiś ca sravan bahiḥ ।
āma eva gudād eti tato alpālpaṃ sa-viḍ-rasaḥ ।।

hidyate pacyate cāntraṃ 'lpālpaḥ sa-viḍ-rasaḥ
tulyaḥ kuṇapa-gandhena picchilaḥ pīta-lohitaḥ ।
śeṣaś cāpūrya jaṭharaṃ jaṭharaṃ ghoram āvahet ।।

vardhayet tad adho nābher āśu caiti jalātma-tām ।
udrikta-doṣa-rūpaṃ ca vyāptaṃ ca śvāsa-tṛḍ-bhramaiḥ ।।

ardhate tad adho nābher yāptaṃ ca śvāsa-tṛḍ-jvaraiḥ
chidrodaram idaṃ prāhuḥ parisrāvīti cāpare ।
pravṛtta-sneha-pānādeḥ sahasāmāmbu-pāyinaḥ ।।

aty-ambu-pānān mandāgneḥ kṣīṇasyāti-kṛśasya vā ।
