ruddhvāmbu-mārgān anilaḥ kaphaś ca jala-mūrchitaḥ ।।

vardhayetāṃ tad evāmbu tat-sthānād udarāśritau ।
tataḥ syād udaraṃ tṛṣṇā-guda-sruti-rujānvitam ।।

-guda-sruti-rujā-yutam
kāsa-śvāsā-ruci-yutaṃ nānā-varṇa-sirā-tatam ।
toya-pūrṇa-dṛti-sparśa-śabda-prakṣobha-vepathu ।।

ānā-varṇa-sirānvitam ānā-varṇa-sirācitam 
nānā-varṇa-sirāvṛtam
dakodaraṃ mahat snigdhaṃ sthiram āvṛtta-nābhi tat ।
upekṣayā ca sarveṣu doṣāḥ sva-sthānataś cyutāḥ ।।

pākād dravā dravī-kuryuḥ saṃdhi-sroto-mukhāny api ।
svedaś ca bāhya-srotaḥsu vihatas tiryag-āsthitaḥ ।।

ākād dravād dravī-kuryuḥ
tad evodakam āpyāyya picchāṃ kuryāt tadā bhavet ।
gurūdaraṃ sthiraṃ vṛttam āhataṃ ca na śabda-vat ।।

mṛdu vyapeta-rājīkaṃ nābhyāṃ spṛṣṭaṃ ca sarpati ।
tad anūdaka-janmāsmin kukṣi-vṛddhis tato adhikam ।।

sirāntardhānam udaka-jaṭharoktaṃ ca lakṣaṇam ।
vāta-pitta-kapha-plīha-saṃnipātodakodaram ।।

kṛcchraṃ yathottaraṃ pakṣāt paraṃ prāyo apare hataḥ ।
sarvaṃ ca jāta-salilaṃ riṣṭoktopadravānvitam ।।

janmanaivodaraṃ sarvaṃ prāyaḥ kṛcchra-tamaṃ matam ।
balinas tad a-jātāmbu yatna-sādhyaṃ navotthitam ।।

nidānasthāna
pitta-pradhānāḥ kupitā yathoktaiḥ kopanair malāḥ ।
tatrānilena balinā kṣiptaṃ pittaṃ hṛdi sthitam ।।

dhamanīr daśa saṃprāpya vyāpnuvat sakalāṃ tanum ।
śleṣma-tvag-rakta-māṃsāni pradūṣyāntaram āśritam ।।

tvaṅ-māṃsayos tat kurute tvaci varṇān pṛthag-vidhān ।
pāṇḍu-hāridra-haritān pāṇḍu-tvaṃ teṣu cādhikam ।।

yato ataḥ pāṇḍur ity uktaḥ sa rogas tena gauravam ।
dhātūnāṃ syāc ca śaithilyam ojasaś ca guṇa-kṣayaḥ ।।

tato alpa-rakta-medasko niḥ-sāraḥ syāc chlathendriyaḥ ।
mṛdyamānair ivāṅgair nā dravatā hṛdayena ca ।।

iḥ-sāraḥ śithilendriyaḥ ravatā hṛdayena vā
śūnākṣi-kūṭaḥ sadanaḥ kopanaḥ ṣṭhīvano alpa-vāk ।
anna-dviṭ śiśira-dveṣī śīrṇa-romā hatānalaḥ ।।

śūnākṣi-kūṭa-vadanaḥ opanaḥ svedano alpa-vāk 
kopanaḥ sadano alpa-vāk
sanna-saktho jvarī śvāsī karṇa-kṣveḍī bhramī śramī ।
sa pañca-dhā pṛthag doṣaiḥ samastair mṛttikādanāt ।।

anna-sakthī jvarī śvāsī
prāg-rūpam asya hṛdaya-spandanaṃ rūkṣa-tā tvaci ।
a-ruciḥ pīta-mūtra-tvaṃ svedā-bhāvo alpa-vahni-tā ।।

sādaḥ śramo anilāt tatra gātra-ruk-toda-kampanam ।
kṛṣṇa-rūkṣāruṇa-sirā-nakha-viṇ-mūtra-netra-tā ।।

śophānāhāsya-vairasya-viṭ-śoṣāḥ pārśva-mūrdha-ruk ।
pittād dharita-pītābha-sirādi-tvaṃ jvaras tamaḥ ।।

tṛṭ-sveda-mūrchā-śītecchā daurgandhyaṃ kaṭu-vaktra-tā ।
varco-bhedo amlako dāhaḥ kaphāc chukla-sirādi-tā ।।

tandrā lavaṇa-vaktra-tvaṃ roma-harṣaḥ svara-kṣayaḥ ।
kāsaś chardiś ca nicayān miśra-liṅgo ati-duḥ-sahaḥ ।।

arṣo romṇāṃ svara-kṣayaḥ
mṛt kaṣāyānilaṃ pittam ūṣarā madhurā kapham ।
dūṣayitvā rasādīṃś ca raukṣyād bhuktaṃ virūkṣya ca ।।

srotāṃsy a-pakvaivāpūrya kuryād ruddhvā ca pūrva-vat ।
pāṇḍu-rogaṃ tataḥ śūna-nābhi-pādāsya-mehanaḥ ।।

purīṣaṃ kṛmi-man muñced bhinnaṃ sāsṛk kaphaṃ naraḥ ।
yaḥ pāṇḍu-rogī seveta pittalaṃ tasya kāmalām ।।

koṣṭha-śākhāśrayāṃ pittaṃ dagdhvāsṛṅ-māṃsam āvahet ।
hāridra-netra-mūtra-tvaṅ-nakha-vaktra-śakṛt-tayā ।।

oṣṭha-śākhāśrayaṃ pittaṃ
dāhā-vipāka-tṛṣṇā-vān bhekābho dur-balendriyaḥ ।
bhavet pittolbaṇasyāsau pāṇḍu-rogād ṛte api ca ।।

upekṣayā ca śophāḍhyā sā kṛcchrā kumbha-kāmalā ।
harita-śyāva-pīta-tvaṃ pāṇḍu-roge yadā bhavet ।।

vāta-pittād bhramas tṛṣṇā strīṣv a-harṣo mṛdur jvaraḥ ।
tandrā balānala-bhraṃśo loḍharaṃ taṃ halīmakam ।।

alasaṃ ceti śaṃsanti teṣāṃ pūrvam upadravāḥ ।
śopha-pradhānāḥ kathitāḥ sa evāto nigadyate ।।

pitta-rakta-kaphān vāyur duṣṭo duṣṭān bahiḥ-sirāḥ ।
nītvā ruddha-gatis tair hi kuryāt tvaṅ-māṃsa-saṃśrayam ।।

utsedhaṃ saṃhataṃ śophaṃ tam āhur nicayād ataḥ ।
sarvaṃ hetu-viśeṣais tu rūpa-bhedān navātmakam ।।

doṣaiḥ pṛthag dvayaiḥ sarvair abhighātād viṣād api ।
dvi-dhā vā nijam āgantuṃ sarvāṅgaikāṅga-jaṃ ca tam ।।

pṛthūnnata-grathita-tā-viśeṣaiś ca tri-dhā viduḥ ।
sāmānya-hetuḥ śophānāṃ doṣa-jānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

vyādhi-karmopavāsādi-kṣīṇasya bhajato drutam ।
ati-mātram athānyasya gurv-amla-snigdha-śītalam ।।

-kṣīṇasya bhajato dravam ti-mātram athānnaṃ ca
lavaṇa-kṣāra-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-śākāmbu svapna-jāgaram ।
mṛd-grāmya-māṃsa-vallūram a-jīrṇa-śrama-maithunam ।।

padāter mārga-gamanaṃ yānena kṣobhiṇāpi vā ।
śvāsa-kāsātisārārśo-jaṭhara-pradara-jvarāḥ ।।

viṣūcy-alasaka-cchardi-garbha-visarpa-pāṇḍavaḥ ।
anye ca mithyopakrāntās tair doṣā vakṣasi sthitāḥ ।।

-garbha-visarpa-pāṇḍu-tā
ūrdhvaṃ śopham adho vastau madhye kurvanti madhya-gāḥ ।
sarvāṅga-gāḥ sarva-gataṃ pratyaṅgeṣu tad-āśrayāḥ ।।

tat-pūrva-rūpaṃ davathuḥ sirāyāmo aṅga-gauravam ।
vātāc chophaś calo rūkṣaḥ khara-romāruṇāsitaḥ ।।

saṃkoca-spanda-harṣārti-toda-bheda-prasupti-mān ।
kṣiprotthāna-śamaḥ śīghram unnamet pīḍitas tanuḥ ।।

snigdhoṣṇa-mardanaiḥ śāmyed rātrāv alpo divā mahān ।
tvak ca sarṣapa-lipteva tasmiṃś cimicimāyate ।।

pīta-raktāsitābhāsaḥ pittād ā-tāmra-roma-kṛt ।
śīghrānusāra-praśamo madhye prāg jāyate tanuḥ ।।

sa-tṛḍ-dāha-jvara-sveda-dava-kleda-mada-bhramaḥ ।
śītābhilāṣī viḍ-bhedī gandhī sparśā-saho mṛduḥ ।।

kaṇḍū-mān pāṇḍu-roma-tvak kaṭhinaḥ śītalo guruḥ ।
snigdhaḥ ślakṣṇaḥ sthiraḥ styāno nidrā-chardy-agni-sāda-kṛt ।।

ākrānto nonnamet kṛcchra-śama-janmā niśā-balaḥ ।
sraven nāsṛk cirāt picchāṃ kuśa-śastrādi-vikṣataḥ ।।

sparśoṣṇa-kāṅkṣī ca kaphād yathā-svaṃ dvandva-jās trayaḥ ।
saṃkarād dhetu-liṅgānāṃ nicayān nicayātmakaḥ ।।

abhighātena śastrādi-ccheda-bheda-kṣatādibhiḥ ।
himāniloda-dhy-anilair bhallāta-kapikacchu-jaiḥ ।।

imānaloda-dhy-anilair
rasaiḥ śūkaiś ca saṃsparśāc chvayathuḥ syād visarpa-vān ।
bhṛśoṣmā lohitābhāsaḥ prāya-śaḥ pitta-lakṣaṇaḥ ।।

viṣa-jaḥ sa-viṣa-prāṇi-parisarpaṇa-mūtraṇāt ।
daṃṣṭrā-danta-nakhāpātād a-viṣa-prāṇinām api ।।

aṃṣṭrā-danta-nakhāghātād
viṇ-mūtra-śukropahata-mala-vad-vastra-saṃkarāt ।
viṣa-vṛkṣānila-sparśād gara-yogāvacūrṇanāt ।।

-mala-vad-vastra-dhāraṇāt
mṛduś calo avalambī ca śīghro dāha-rujā-karaḥ ।
navo an-upadravaḥ śophaḥ sādhyo a-sādhyaḥ pureritaḥ ।।

syād visarpo abhighātāntair doṣair dūṣyaiś ca śopha-vat ।
try-adhiṣṭhānaṃ ca taṃ prāhur bāhyāntar-ubhayāśrayāt ।।

yathottaraṃ ca duḥ-sādhyās tatra doṣā yathā-yatham ।
prakopaṇaiḥ prakupitā viśeṣeṇa vidāhibhiḥ ।।

dehe śīghraṃ visarpanti te antar antaḥ-sthitā bahiḥ ।
bahiḥ-sthā dvitaye dvi-sthā vidyāt tatrāntar-āśrayam ।।

marmopatāpāt saṃmohād ayanānāṃ vighaṭṭanāt ।
tṛṣṇāti-yogād vegānāṃ viṣamaṃ ca pravartanāt ।।

armopaghātāt saṃmohād iṣamāc ca pravartanāt
āśu cāgni-bala-bhraṃśād ato bāhyaṃ viparyayāt ।
tatra vātāt parīsarpo vāta-jvara-sama-vyathaḥ ।।

śopha-sphuraṇa-nistoda-bhedāyāmārti-harṣa-vān ।
pittād druta-gatiḥ pitta-jvara-liṅgo ati-lohitaḥ ।।

kaphāt kaṇḍū-yutaḥ snigdhaḥ kapha-jvara-samāna-ruk ।
sva-doṣa-liṅgaiś cīyante sarve sphoṭair upekṣitāḥ ।।

te pakva-bhinnāḥ svaṃ svaṃ ca bibhrati vraṇa-lakṣaṇam ।
vāta-pittāj jvara-cchardi-mūrchātīsāra-tṛḍ-bhramaiḥ ।।

asthi-bhedāgni-sadana-tamakā-rocakair yutaḥ ।
karoti sarvam aṅgaṃ ca dīptāṅgārāvakīrṇa-vat ।।

yaṃ yaṃ deśaṃ visarpaś ca visarpati bhavet sa saḥ ।
śāntāṅgārāsito nīlo rakto vāśu ca cīyate ।।

agni-dagdha iva sphoṭaiḥ śīghra-ga-tvād drutaṃ ca saḥ ।
marmānusārī vīsarpaḥ syād vāto ati-balas tataḥ ।।

vyathetāṅgaṃ haret saṃjñāṃ nidrāṃ ca śvāsam īrayet ।
hidhmāṃ ca sa gato avasthām īdṛśīṃ labhate na nā ।।

kva-cic charmā-rati-grasto bhūmi-śayyāsanādiṣu ।
ceṣṭamānas tataḥ kliṣṭo mano-deha-śramodbhavām ।।

duṣ-prabodho aśnute nidrāṃ so agni-visarpa ucyate ।
kaphena ruddhaḥ pavano bhittvā taṃ bahu-dhā kapham ।।

raktaṃ vā vṛddha-raktasya tvak-sirā-snāva-māṃsa-gam ।
dūṣayitvā ca dīrghāṇu-vṛtta-sthūla-kharātmanām ।।

granthīnāṃ kurute mālāṃ raktānāṃ tīvra-rug-jvarām ।
śvāsa-kāsātisārāsya-śoṣa-hidhmā-vami-bhramaiḥ ।।

moha-vaivarṇya-mūrchāṅga-bhaṅgāgni-sadanair yutām ।
ity ayaṃ granthi-vīsarpaḥ kapha-māruta-kopa-jaḥ ।।

kapha-pittāj jvaraḥ stambho nidrā-tandrā-śiro-rujaḥ ।
aṅgāvasāda-vikṣepa-pralāpā-rocaka-bhramāḥ ।।

mūrchāgni-hānir bhedo asthnāṃ pipāsendriya-gauravam ।
āmopaveśanaṃ lepaḥ srotasāṃ sa ca sarpati ।।

prāyeṇāmāśaye gṛhṇann eka-deśaṃ na cāti-ruk ।
piṭikair avakīrṇo ati-pīta-lohita-pāṇḍuraiḥ ।।

mecakābho asitaḥ snigdho malinaḥ śopha-vān guruḥ ।
gambhīra-pākaḥ prājyoṣmā spṛṣṭaḥ klinno avadīryate ।।

ecakābho asita-snigdho
paṅka-vac-chīrṇa-māṃsaś ca spaṣṭa-snāyu-sirā-gaṇaḥ ।
śava-gandhiś ca vīsarpaṃ kardamākhyam uśanti tam ।।

sarva-jo lakṣaṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ sarva-dhātv-atisarpaṇaḥ ।
bāhya-hetoḥ kṣatāt kruddhaḥ sa-raktaṃ pittam īrayan ।।

arva-dhātv-abhisarpaṇaḥ
visarpaṃ mārutaḥ kuryāt kulattha-sadṛśaiś citam ।
sphoṭaiḥ śopha-jvara-rujā-dāhāḍhyaṃ śyāva-lohitam ।।

pṛthag doṣais trayaḥ sādhyā dvandva-jāś cān-upadravāḥ ।
a-sādhyau kṣata-sarvotthau sarve cākrānta-marmakāḥ ।।
śīrṇa-snāyu-sirā-māṃsāḥ praklinnāḥ śava-gandhayaḥ ।।
nidānasthāna
mithyāhāra-vihāreṇa viśeṣeṇa virodhinā ।
sādhu-nindā-vadhānya-sva-haraṇādyaiś ca sevitaiḥ ।।

pāpmabhiḥ karmabhiḥ sadyaḥ prāktanair veritā malāḥ ।
sirāḥ prapadya tiryag-gās tvag-lasīkāsṛg-āmiṣam ।।

rāktanaiḥ preritā malāḥ
dūṣayanti ślathī-kṛtya niścarantas tato bahiḥ ।
tvacaḥ kurvanti vaivarṇyaṃ duṣṭāḥ kuṣṭham uśanti tat ।।

ūṣayantaḥ ślathī-kṛtya
kālenopekṣitaṃ yasmāt sarvaṃ kuṣṇāti tad vapuḥ ।
prapadya dhātūn vyāpyāntaḥ sarvān saṃkledya cāvahet ।।

sa-sveda-kleda-saṃkothān kṛmīn sūkṣmān su-dāruṇān ।
roma-tvak-snāyu-dhamanī-taruṇāsthīni yaiḥ kramāt ।।

bhakṣayec chvitram asmāc ca kuṣṭha-bāhyam udāhṛtam ।
kuṣṭhāni sapta-dhā doṣaiḥ pṛthaṅ miśraiḥ samāgataiḥ ।।

ṛthag dvandvaiḥ samāgataiḥ
sarveṣv api tri-doṣeṣu vyapadeśo adhika-tvataḥ ।
vātena kuṣṭhaṃ kāpālaṃ pittād audumbaraṃ kaphāt ।।

maṇḍalākhyaṃ vicarcī ca ṛkṣākhyaṃ vāta-pitta-jam ।
carmaika-kuṣṭha-kiṭibha-sidhmālasa-vipādikāḥ ।।

ṛkṣākṣaṃ vāta-pitta-jam
vāta-śleṣmodbhavāḥ śleṣma-pittād dadrū-śatāruṣī ।
puṇḍarīkaṃ sa-visphoṭaṃ pāmā carma-dalaṃ tathā ।।

sarvaiḥ syāt kākaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ trikaṃ dadru sa-kākaṇam ।
puṇḍarīkarkṣa-jihve ca mahā-kuṣṭhāni sapta tu ।।

rikaṃ dadrūḥ sa-kākaṇā uṇḍarīkarśya-jihve ca
ati-ślakṣṇa-khara-sparśa-khedā-sveda-vi-varṇa-tāḥ ।
dāhaḥ kaṇḍūs tvaci svāpas todaḥ koṭhonnatiḥ śramaḥ ।।

vraṇānām adhikaṃ śūlaṃ śīghrotpattiś cira-sthitiḥ ।
rūḍhānām api rūkṣa-tvaṃ nimitte alpe api kopanam ।।

roma-harṣo asṛjaḥ kārṣṇyam kuṣṭha-lakṣaṇam agra-jam ।
kṛṣṇāruṇa-kapālābhaṃ rūkṣaṃ suptaṃ kharaṃ tanu ।।

vistṛtā-sama-pary-antaṃ hṛṣitair romabhiś citam ।
todāḍhyam alpa-kaṇḍūkaṃ kāpālaṃ śīghra-sarpi ca ।।

ūṣitair romabhiś citam
pakvodumbara-tāmra-tvag-roma gaura-sirā-citam ।
bahalaṃ bahala-kleda-raktaṃ dāha-rujādhikam ।।

-roma gaura-sirā-tatam ahulaṃ bahula-kleda-
āśūtthānāvadaraṇa-kṛmi vidyād udumbaram ।
sthiraṃ styānaṃ guru snigdhaṃ śveta-raktam an-āśu-gam ।।

anyo-'nya-saktam utsannaṃ bahu-kaṇḍū-sruti-krimi ।
ślakṣṇa-pītābha-pary-antaṃ maṇḍalaṃ parimaṇḍalam ।।

nyo-'nya-saktam ucchūnaṃ nyo-'nya-saktam utsaṅgaṃ
sa-kaṇḍū-piṭikā śyāvā lasīkāḍhyā vicarcikā ।
paruṣaṃ tanu raktāntam antaḥ-śyāvaṃ samunnatam ।।

sa-toda-dāha-ruk-kledaṃ karkaśaiḥ piṭikaiś citam ।
ṛkṣa-jihvākṛti proktam ṛkṣa-jihvaṃ bahu-krimi ।।

ṛśya-jihvākṛti proktam ṛśya-jihvaṃ bahu-krimi
hasti-carma-khara-sparśaṃ carmaikākhyaṃ mahāśrayam ।
a-svedaṃ matsya-śakala-saṃnibhaṃ kiṭibhaṃ punaḥ ।।

rūkṣaṃ kiṇa-khara-sparśaṃ kaṇḍū-mat paruṣāsitam ।
sidhmaṃ rūkṣaṃ bahiḥ snigdham antar ghṛṣṭaṃ rajaḥ kiret ।।

ślakṣṇa-sparśaṃ tanu śveta-tāmraṃ daugdhika-puṣpa-vat ।
prāyeṇa cordhva-kāye syād gaṇḍaiḥ kaṇḍū-yutaiś citam ।।

raktair alasakaṃ pāṇi-pāda-dāryo vipādikāḥ ।
tīvrārtyo manda-kaṇḍvaś ca sa-rāga-piṭikācitāḥ ।।

dīrgha-pratānā dūrvā-vad atasī-kusuma-cchaviḥ ।
utsanna-maṇḍalā dadrūḥ kaṇḍū-maty anuṣaṅgiṇī ।।

sthūla-mūlaṃ sa-dāhārti rakta-śyāvaṃ bahu-vraṇam ।
śatāruḥ kleda-jantv-āḍhyaṃ prāya-śaḥ parva-janma ca ।।

raktāntam antarā pāṇḍu kaṇḍū-dāha-rujānvitam ।
sotsedham ācitaṃ raktaiḥ padma-pattram ivāṃśubhiḥ ।।

ghana-bhūri-lasīkāsṛk-prāyam āśu vibhedi ca ।
puṇḍarīkaṃ tanu-tvagbhiś citaṃ sphoṭaiḥ sitāruṇaiḥ ।।

visphoṭaṃ piṭikāḥ pāmā kaṇḍū-kleda-rujādhikāḥ ।
sūkṣmāḥ śyāvāruṇā bahvyaḥ prāyaḥ sphik-pāṇi-kūrpare ।।

sa-sphoṭam a-sparśa-sahaṃ kaṇḍūṣā-toda-dāha-vat ।
raktaṃ dalac carma-dalaṃ kākaṇaṃ tīvra-dāha-ruk ।।

pūrvaṃ raktaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca kākaṇantī-phalopamam ।
kuṣṭha-liṅgair yutaṃ sarvair naika-varṇaṃ tato bhavet ।।

doṣa-bhedīya-vihitair ādiśel liṅga-karmabhiḥ ।
kuṣṭheṣu doṣolbaṇa-tāṃ sarva-doṣolbaṇaṃ tyajet ।।

riṣṭoktaṃ yac ca yac cāsthi-majja-śukra-samāśrayam ।
yāpyaṃ medo-gataṃ kṛcchraṃ pitta-dvandvāsra-māṃsa-gam ।।

a-kṛcchraṃ kapha-vātāḍhyaṃ tvak-stham eka-malaṃ ca yat ।
tatra tvaci sthite kuṣṭhe toda-vaivarṇya-rūkṣa-tāḥ ।।

sveda-svāpa-śvayathavaḥ śoṇite piśite punaḥ ।
pāṇi-pādāśritāḥ sphoṭāḥ kledaḥ saṃdhiṣu cādhikam ।।

kauṇyaṃ gati-kṣayo aṅgānāṃ dalanaṃ syāc ca medasi ।
nāsā-bhaṅgo asthi-majja-sthe netra-rāgaḥ svara-kṣayaḥ ।।

kṣate ca kṛmayaḥ śukre sva-dārāpatya-bādhanam ।
yathā-pūrvaṃ ca sarvāṇi syur liṅgāny asṛg-ādiṣu ।।

va-dārāpatya-dhāvanam
kuṣṭhaika-saṃbhavaṃ śvitraṃ kilāsaṃ dāruṇaṃ ca tat ।
nirdiṣṭam a-parisrāvi tri-dhātūdbhava-saṃśrayam ।।

ilāsaṃ cāruṇaṃ ca tat
vātād rūkṣāruṇaṃ pittāt tāmraṃ kamala-pattra-vat ।
sa-dāhaṃ roma-vidhvaṃsi kaphāc chvetaṃ ghanaṃ guru ।।

sa-kaṇḍu ca kramād rakta-māṃsa-medaḥsu cādiśet ।
varṇenaivedṛg ubhayaṃ kṛcchraṃ tac cottarottaram ।।

a-śukla-romā-bahalam a-saṃsṛṣṭaṃ mitho navam ।
an-agni-dagdha-jaṃ sādhyaṃ śvitraṃ varjyam ato anya-thā ।।

-śukla-romā-bahulam -saṃsṛṣṭam atho navam
guhya-pāṇi-talauṣṭheṣu jātam apy a-ciran-tanam ।
sparśaikāhāra-śayyādi-sevanāt prāya-śo gadāḥ ।।

sarve saṃcāriṇo netra-tvag-vikārā viśeṣataḥ ।
kṛmayas tu dvi-dhā proktā bāhyābhyantara-bhedataḥ ।।

bahir-mala-kaphāsṛg-viḍ-janma-bhedāc catur-vidhāḥ ।
nāmato viṃśati-vidhā bāhyās tatrā-mṛjodbhavāḥ ।।

āhyās tatra malodbhavāḥ āhyās tatrāsṛg-udbhavāḥ
tila-pramāṇa-saṃsthāna-varṇāḥ keśāmbarāśrayāḥ ।
bahu-pādāś ca sūkṣmāś ca yūkā likṣāś ca nāmataḥ ।।

dvi-dhā te koṭha-piṭikā-kaṇḍū-gaṇḍān prakurvate ।
kuṣṭhaika-hetavo antar-jāḥ śleṣma-jās teṣu cādhikam ।।

madhurānna-guḍa-kṣīra-dadhi-saktu-navaudanaiḥ ।
śakṛj-jā bahu-viḍ-dhānya-parṇa-śākolakādibhiḥ ।।

adhurāmla-guḍa-kṣīra- -parṇa-śākaukulādibhiḥ
kaphād āmāśaye jātā vṛddhāḥ sarpanti sarvataḥ ।
pṛthu-bradhna-nibhāḥ ke-cit ke-cid gaṇḍū-padopamāḥ ।।

rūḍha-dhānyāṅkurākārās tanu-dīrghās tathāṇavaḥ ।
śvetās tāmrāvabhāsāś ca nāmataḥ sapta-dhā tu te ।।

antrādā udarāveṣṭā hṛdayādā mahā-kuhāḥ ।
kuravo darbha-kusumāḥ su-gandhās te ca kurvate ।।

ntrādā udarāviṣṭā ṛdayādā mahā-ruhāḥ uravo 
darbha-kusumāḥ
hṛl-lāsam āsya-sravaṇam a-vipākam a-rocakam ।
mūrchā-chardi-jvarānāha-kārśya-kṣavathu-pīnasān ।।

rakta-vāhi-sirotthānā rakta-jā jantavo aṇavaḥ ।
a-pādā vṛtta-tāmrāś ca saukṣmyāt ke-cid a-darśanāḥ ।।

akta-vāhi-sirā-sthānād akta-vāhi-sirā-sthānā
keśādā roma-vidhvaṃsā roma-dvīpā udumbarāḥ ।
ṣaṭ te kuṣṭhaika-karmāṇaḥ saha-saurasa-mātaraḥ ।।

c saha-jā rasa-mātaraḥ
pakvāśaye purīṣotthā jāyante adho-visarpiṇaḥ ।
vṛddhāḥ santo bhaveyuś ca te yadāmāśayon-mukhāḥ ।।

ṛddhās te syur bhaveyuś ca
tadāsyodgāra-niḥśvāsā viḍ-gandhānuvidhāyinaḥ ।
pṛthu-vṛtta-tanu-sthūlāḥ śyāva-pīta-sitāsitāḥ ।।

te pañca nāmnā kṛmayaḥ kakeruka-makerukāḥ ।
sausurādāḥ sulūnākhyā lelihā janayanti ca ।।

ausurādāḥ śalūnākhyā
viḍ-bheda-śūla-viṣṭambha-kārśya-pāruṣya-pāṇḍu-tāḥ ।
roma-harṣāgni-sadana-guda-kaṇḍūr vinirgamāt ।।

-guda-kaṇḍūr vinirgatāḥ -guda-kaṇḍūr vi-mārga-gāḥ

nidānasthāna
sarvārthān-artha-karaṇe viśvasyāsyaika-kāraṇam ।
a-duṣṭa-duṣṭaḥ pavanaḥ śarīrasya viśeṣataḥ ।।

sa viśva-karmā viśvātmā viśva-rūpaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
sraṣṭā dhātā vibhur viṣṇuḥ saṃhartā mṛtyur antakaḥ ।।

tad-a-duṣṭau prayatnena yatitavyam ataḥ sadā ।
tasyoktaṃ doṣa-vijñāne karma prākṛta-vaikṛtam ।।

samāsād vyāsato doṣa-bhedīye nāma dhāma ca ।
praty-ekaṃ pañca-dhā cāro vyāpāraś ceha vaikṛtam ।।

tasyocyate vibhāgena sa-nidānaṃ sa-lakṣaṇam ।
dhātu-kṣaya-karair vāyuḥ kupyaty ati-niṣevitaiḥ ।।

a-saṃkhyam api saṃkhyāya yad aśītyā pureritam ab ।।

yathāśīty apareritam
caran srotaḥsu rikteṣu bhṛśaṃ tāny eva pūrayan ।
tebhyo anya-doṣa-pūrṇebhyaḥ prāpya vāvaraṇaṃ balī ।।

tatra pakvāśaye kruddhaḥ śūlānāhāntra-kūjanam ।
mala-rodhāśma-vardhmārśas-trika-pṛṣṭha-kaṭī-graham ।।

karoty adhara-kāye ca tāṃs tān kṛcchrān upadravān ।
āmāśaye tṛḍ-vamathu-śvāsa-kāsa-viṣūcikāḥ ।।

aroty adhara-kāyeṣu
kaṇṭhoparodham udgārān vyādhīn ūrdhvaṃ ca nābhitaḥ ।
śrotrādiṣv indriya-vadhaṃ tvaci sphuṭana-rūkṣa-te ।।

rakte tīvrā rujaḥ svāpaṃ tāpaṃ rāgaṃ vi-varṇa-tām ।
arūṃṣy annasya viṣṭambham a-ruciṃ kṛśa-tāṃ bhramam ।।

rūṃṣy aṅgasya viṣṭambham
māṃsa-medo-gato granthīṃs todāḍhyān karkaśāñ chramam ।
gurv aṅgaṃ cāti-ruk stabdhaṃ muṣṭi-daṇḍa-hatopamam ।।

odāḍhyān karkaśāñ chramān odāḍhyān karkaśān bhṛśam
asthi-sthaḥ sakthi-saṃdhy-asthi-śūlaṃ tīvraṃ bala-kṣayam ।
majja-stho asthiṣu sauṣiryam a-svapnaṃ saṃtatāṃ rujam ।।

-svapnaṃ stabdha-tāṃ rujam
śukrasya śīghram utsargaṃ saṅgaṃ vikṛtim eva vā ।
tad-vad garbhasya śukra-sthaḥ sirāsv ādhmāna-rikta-te ।।

tat-sthaḥ snāva-sthitaḥ kuryād gṛdhrasy-āyāma-kubja-tāḥ ।
vāta-pūrṇa-dṛti-sparśaṃ śophaṃ saṃdhi-gato anilaḥ ।।

ṛdhrasy-āyāma-kubja-tām
prasāraṇākuñcanayoḥ pravṛttiṃ ca sa-vedanām ।
sarvāṅga-saṃśrayas toda-bheda-sphuraṇa-bhañjanam ।।

stambhanākṣepaṇa-svāpa-saṃdhy-ākuñcana-kampanam ।
yadā tu dhamanīḥ sarvāḥ kruddho abhyeti muhur muhuḥ ।।

tadāṅgam ākṣipaty eṣa vyādhir ākṣepakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
adhaḥ pratihato vāyur vrajann ūrdhvaṃ hṛd-āśritāḥ ।।

rajann ūrdhvaṃ hṛd-āśrayāḥ
nāḍīḥ praviśya hṛdayaṃ śiraḥ śaṅkhau ca pīḍayan ।
ākṣipet parito gātraṃ dhanur-vac cāsya nāmayet ।।

śiraḥ śaṅkhau ca pīḍayet
kṛcchrād ucchvasiti stabdha-srasta-mīlita-dṛk tataḥ ।
kapota iva kūjec ca niḥ-saṃjñaḥ so apatantrakaḥ ।।

sa eva cāpatānākyho mukte tu marutā hṛdi ।
aśnuvīta muhuḥ svāsthyaṃ muhur a-svāsthyam āvṛte ।।

śnuvīta iva svāsthyaṃ
garbha-pāta-samutpannaḥ śoṇitāti-sravotthitaḥ ।
abhighāta-samutthaś ca duś-cikitsya-tamo hi saḥ ।।

manye saṃstabhya vāto antar āyacchan dhamanīr yadā ।
vyāpnoti sakalaṃ dehaṃ jatrur āyamyate tadā ।।

āgacchan dhamanīr yadā
antar dhanur ivāṅgaṃ ca vegaiḥ stambhaṃ ca netrayoḥ ।
karoti jṛmbhāṃ daśanaṃ daśanānāṃ kaphodvamam ।।

pārśvayor vedanāṃ vākya-hanu-pṛṣṭha-śiro-graham ।
antar-āyāma ity eṣa bāhyāyāmaś ca tad-vidhaḥ ।।

dehasya bahir-āyāmāt pṛṣṭhato nīyate śiraḥ ।
uraś cotkṣipyate tatra kandharā cāvamṛdyate ।।

ṛṣṭhato hriyate śiraḥ
danteṣv āsye ca vaivarṇyaṃ prasvedaḥ srasta-gātra-tā ।
bāhyāyāmaṃ dhanuḥ-ṣkambhaṃ bruvate veginaṃ ca tam ।।

āhyāyāmaṃ dhanuḥ-stambhaṃ
vraṇaṃ marmāśritaṃ prāpya samīraṇa-samīraṇāt ।
vyāyacchanti tanuṃ doṣāḥ sarvām ā-pāda-mastakam ।।

raṇaṃ marmāśrayaṃ prāpya
tṛṣyataḥ pāṇḍu-gātrasya vraṇāyāmaḥ sa varjitaḥ ।
gate vege bhavet svāsthyaṃ sarveṣv ākṣepakeṣu ca ।।

arveṣv ākṣepakeṣu tu
jihvāti-lekhanāc chuṣka-bhakṣaṇād abhighātataḥ ।
kupito hanu-mūla-sthaḥ sraṃsayitvānilo hanū ।।

karoti vivṛtāsya-tvam atha-vā saṃvṛtāsya-tām ।
hanu-sraṃsaḥ sa tena syāt kṛcchrāc carvaṇa-bhāṣaṇam ।।

vāg-vāhinī-sirā-saṃstho jihvāṃ stambhayate anilaḥ ।
jihvā-stambhaḥ sa tenānna-pāna-vākyeṣv an-īśa-tā ।।

śirasā bhāra-haraṇād ati-hāsya-prabhāṣaṇāt ।
uttrāsa-vaktra-kṣavathoḥ khara-kārmuka-karṣaṇāt ।।

cchvāsa-vakra-kṣavathu- ttrāsa-vaktra-kṣavathu- 
-khara-kārmuka-karṣaṇāt
viṣamād upadhānāc ca kaṭhinānāṃ ca carvaṇāt ।
vāyur vivṛddhas tais taiś ca vātalair ūrdhvam āsthitaḥ ।।

vakrī-karoti vaktrārdham uktaṃ hasitam īkṣitam ।
tato asya kampate mūrdhā vāk-saṅgaḥ stabdha-netra-tā ।।

āg-bhaṅgaḥ stabdha-netra-tā
danta-cālaḥ svara-bhraṃśaḥ śruti-hāniḥ kṣava-grahaḥ ।
gandhā-jñānaṃ smṛter mohas trāsaḥ suptasya jāyate ।।

niṣṭhīvaḥ pārśvato yāyād ekasyākṣṇo nimīlanam ।
jatror ūrdhvaṃ rujā tīvrā śarīrārdhe adhare api vā ।।

tam āhur arditaṃ ke-cid ekāyāmam athāpare ।
raktam āśritya pavanaḥ kuryān mūrdha-dharāḥ sirāḥ ।।

rūkṣāḥ sa-vedanāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ so a-sādhyaḥ syāt sirā-grahaḥ ।
gṛhītvārdhaṃ tanor vāyuḥ sirāḥ snāyūr viśoṣya ca ।।

pakṣam anya-taraṃ hanti saṃdhi-bandhān vimokṣayan ।
kṛtsno ardha-kāyas tasya syād a-karmaṇyo vi-cetanaḥ ।।

ekāṅga-rogaṃ taṃ ke-cid anye pakṣa-vadhaṃ viduḥ ।
sarvāṅga-rogaṃ tad-vac ca sarva-kāyāśrite anile ।।

śuddha-vāta-hataḥ pakṣaḥ kṛcchra-sādhya-tamo mataḥ ।
kṛcchras tv anyena saṃsṛṣṭo vivarjyaḥ kṣaya-hetukaḥ ।।

āma-baddhāyanaḥ kuryāt saṃsthabhyāṅgaṃ kaphānvitaḥ ।
a-sādhyaṃ hata-sarvehaṃ daṇḍa-vad daṇḍakaṃ marut ।।

aṃsa-mūla-sthito vāyuḥ sirāḥ saṃkocya tatra-gāḥ ।
bāhu-praspandita-haraṃ janayaty ava-bāhukam ।।

talaṃ praty aṅgulīnāṃ yā kaṇḍarā bāhu-pṛṣṭhataḥ ।
bāhu-ceṣṭāpaharaṇī viśvācī nāma sā smṛtā ।।

āhvoḥ karma-kṣaya-karī
vāyuḥ kaṭyāṃ sthitaḥ sakthnaḥ kaṇḍarām ākṣiped yadā ।
tadā khañjo bhavej jantuḥ paṅguḥ sakthnor dvayor api ।।

kampate gamanārambhe khañjann iva ca yāti yaḥ ।
kalāya-khañjaṃ taṃ vidyān mukta-saṃdhi-prabandhanam ।।

śītoṣṇa-drava-saṃśuṣka-guru-snigdhair niṣevitaiḥ ।
jīrṇā-jīrṇe tathāyāsa-saṃkṣobha-svapna-jāgaraiḥ ।।

sa-śleṣma-medaḥ-pavanam āmam aty-artha-saṃcitam ।
abhibhūyetaraṃ doṣam ūrū cet pratipadyate ।।

sakthy-asthīni prapūryāntaḥ śleṣmaṇā stimitena tat ।
tadā skabhnāti tenorū stabdhau śītāvacetanau ।।

adā skandati tenorū adā skannāti tenorū
parakīyāv iva gurū syātām ati-bhṛśa-vyathau ।
dhyānāṅga-marda-staimitya-tandrā-chardy-a-ruci-jvaraiḥ ।।

saṃyutau pāda-sadana-kṛcchroddharaṇa-suptibhiḥ ।
tam ūru-stambham ity āhur āḍhya-vātam athāpare ।।

aṃyuktau pāda-sadana-
vāta-śoṇita-jaḥ śopho jānu-madhye mahā-rujaḥ ।
jñeyaḥ kroṣṭuka-śīrṣaś ca sthūlaḥ kroṣṭuka-śīrṣa-vat ।।

thūlaḥ kroṣṭuka-mūrdha-vat
ruk pāde viṣama-nyaste śramād vā jāyate yadā ।
vātena gulpham āśritya tam āhur vāta-kaṇṭakam ।।

pārṣṇiṃ praty aṅgulīnāṃ yā kaṇḍarā mārutārditā ।
sakthy-utkṣepaṃ nigṛhṇāti gṛdhrasīṃ tāṃ pracakṣate ।।

viśvācī gṛdhrasī coktā khallis tīvra-rujānvite ।
hṛṣyete caraṇau yasya bhavetāṃ ca prasupta-vat ।।

hallis tīvra-rujānvitā
pāda-harṣaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ kapha-māruta-kopa-jaḥ ।
pādayoḥ kurute dāhaṃ pittāsṛk-sahito anilaḥ ।।
viśeṣataś caṅkramite pāda-dāhaṃ tam ādiśet ।।
ū̆viśeṣataś caṅkramataḥ

nidānasthāna
vidāhy annaṃ viruddhaṃ ca tat tac cāsṛk-pradūṣaṇam ।
bhajatāṃ vidhi-hīnaṃ ca svapna-jāgara-maithunam ।।

at tathāsṛk-pradūṣaṇam
prāyeṇa su-kumārāṇām a-caṅkramaṇa-śīlinām ।
abhighātād a-śuddheś ca nṛṇām asṛji dūṣite ।।

vātalaiḥ śītalair vāyur vṛddhaḥ kruddho vi-mārga-gaḥ ।
tādṛśaivāsṛjā ruddhaḥ prāk tad eva pradūṣayet ।।

ādṛśenāsṛjā ruddhaḥ
āḍhya-rogaṃ khuḍaṃ vāta-balāsaṃ vāta-śoṇitam ।
tad āhur nāmabhis tac ca pūrvaṃ pādau pradhāvati ।।

-palāśaṃ vāta-śoṇitam
viśeṣād yāna-yānād yaiḥ pralambau tasya lakṣaṇam ।
bhaviṣyataḥ kuṣṭha-samaṃ tathā sādaḥ ślathāṅga-tā ।।

jānu-jaṅghoru-kaṭy-aṃsa-hasta-pādāṅga-saṃdhiṣu ।
kaṇḍū-sphuraṇa-nistoda-bheda-gaurava-supta-tāḥ ।।

bhūtvā bhūtvā praṇaśyanti muhur āvir-bhavanti ca ।
pādayor mūlam āsthāya kadā-cid dhastayor api ।।

ākhor iva viṣaṃ kruddhaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dehaṃ vidhāvati ।
tvaṅ-māṃsāśrayam uttānaṃ tat pūrvaṃ jāyate tataḥ ।।

kālāntareṇa gambhīraṃ sarvān dhātūn abhidravat ।
kaṇḍv-ādi-saṃyutottāne tvak tāmrā śyāva-lohitā ।।

sāyāmā bhṛśa-dāhoṣā gambhīre adhika-pūrva-ruk ।
śvayathur grathitaḥ pākī vāyuḥ saṃdhy-asthi-majjasu ।।

chindann iva caraty antar vakrī-kurvaṃś ca vega-vān ।
karoti khañjaṃ paṅguṃ vā śarīre sarvataś caran ।।

hindann iva carann antar
vāte adhike adhikaṃ tatra śūla-sphuraṇa-todanam ।
śophasya raukṣya-kṛṣṇa-tva-śyāva-tā-vṛddhi-hānayaḥ ।।

dhamany-aṅguli-saṃdhīnāṃ saṃkoco aṅga-graho ati-ruk ।
śīta-dveṣān-upaśayau stambha-vepathu-suptayaḥ ।।

rakte śopho ati-ruk todas tāmraś cimicimāyate ।
snigdha-rūkṣaiḥ śamaṃ naiti kaṇḍū-kleda-samanvitaḥ ।।

pitte vidāhaḥ saṃmohaḥ svedo mūrchā madaḥ sa-tṛṭ ।
sparśā-kṣama-tvaṃ rug rāgaḥ śophaḥ pāko bhṛśoṣma-tā ।।

kaphe staimitya-guru-tā-supti-snigdha-tva-śita-tāḥ ।
kaṇḍūr mandā ca rug dvandva-sarva-liṅgaṃ ca saṃkare ।।

eka-doṣānugaṃ sādhyaṃ navaṃ yāpyaṃ dvi-doṣa-jam ।
tri-doṣa-jaṃ tyajet srāvi stabdham arbuda-kāri ca ।।

ri-doṣaṃ tat tyajet srāvi
rakta-mārgaṃ nihatyāśu śākhā-saṃdhiṣu mārutaḥ ।
niviśyānyo-'nyam āvārya vedanābhir haraty asūn ।।

akta-mārgaṃ nihanty āśu
vāyau pañcātmake prāṇo raukṣya-vyāyāma-laṅghanaiḥ ।
aty-āhārābhighātādhva-vegodīraṇa-dhāraṇaiḥ ।।

ūkṣa-vyāyāma-laṅghanaiḥ
kupitaś cakṣur-ādīnām upaghātaṃ pravartayet ।
pīnasārdita-tṛṭ-kāsa-śvāsādīṃś cāmayān bahūn ।।

udānaḥ kṣavathūdgāra-cchardi-nidrā-vidhāraṇaiḥ ।
guru-bhārāti-rudita-hāsyādyair vikṛto gadān ।।

-cchardi-nidrāvadhāraṇaiḥ
kaṇṭha-rodha-mano-bhraṃśa-cchardy-a-rocaka-pīnasān ।
kuryāc ca gala-gaṇḍādīṃs tāṃs tāñ jatrūrdhva-saṃśrayān ।।

vyāno ati-gamana-dhyāna-krīḍā-viṣama-ceṣṭitaiḥ ।
virodhi-rūkṣa-bhī-harṣa-viṣādādyaiś ca dūṣitaḥ ।।

yāno ati-gamana-sthāna-
puṃs-tvotsāha-bala-bhraṃśa-śopha-cittotplava-jvarān ।
sarvāṅga-roga-nistoda-roma-harṣāṅga-supta-tāḥ ।।

-roma-harṣāṅga-supti-tāḥ
kuṣṭhaṃ visarpam anyāṃś ca kuryāt sarvāṅga-gān gadān ।
samāno viṣamā-jīrṇa-śīta-saṃkīrṇa-bhojanaiḥ ।।

karoty a-kāla-śayana-jāgarādyaiś ca dūṣitaḥ ।
śūla-gulma-grahaṇy-ādīn pakvāmāśaya-jān gadān ।।

apāno rūkṣa-gurv-anna-vegāghātāti-vāhanaiḥ ।
yāna-yānāsana-sthāna-caṅkramaiś cāti-sevitaiḥ ।।

-vega-ghātāti-vāhanaiḥ
kupitaḥ kurute rogān kṛcchrān pakvāśayāśrayān ।
mūtra-śukra-pradoṣārśo-guda-bhraṃśādikān bahūn ।।

sarvaṃ ca mārutaṃ sāmaṃ tandrā-staimitya-gauravaiḥ ।
snigdha-tvā-rocakālasya-śaitya-śophāgni-hānibhiḥ ।।

kaṭu-rūkṣābhilāṣeṇa tad-vidhopaśayena ca ।
yuktaṃ vidyān nir-āmaṃ tu tandrādīnāṃ viparyayāt ।।

vāyor āvaraṇaṃ cāto bahu-bhedaṃ pravakṣyate ।
liṅgaṃ pittāvṛte dāhas tṛṣṇā śūlaṃ bhramas tamaḥ ।।

ahu-bhedaṃ pracakṣyate
kaṭukoṣṇāmla-lavaṇair vidāhaḥ śīta-kāma-tā ।
śaitya-gaurava-śūlāni kaṭv-ādy-upaśayo adhikam ।।

laṅghanāyāsa-rūkṣoṣṇa-kāma-tā ca kaphāvṛte ।
raktāvṛte sa-dāhārtis tvaṅ-māṃsāntara-jā bhṛśam ।।

bhavec ca rāgī śvayathur jāyante maṇḍalāni ca ।
māṃsena kaṭhinaḥ śopho vi-varṇaḥ piṭikās tathā ।।

harṣaḥ pipīlikānāṃ ca saṃcāra iva jāyate ।
calaḥ snigdho mṛduḥ śītaḥ śopho gātreṣv a-rocakaḥ ।।

arṣaḥ pipīlikādīnāṃ
āḍhya-vāta iti jñeyaḥ sa kṛcchro medasāvṛte ।
sparśam asthy-āvṛte aty-uṣṇaṃ pīḍanaṃ cābhinandati ।।

sūcyeva tudyate aty-artham aṅgaṃ sīdati śūlyate ।
majjāvṛte vinamanaṃ jṛmbhaṇaṃ pariveṣṭanam ।।

śūlaṃ ca pīḍyamānena pāṇibhyāṃ labhate sukham ।
śukrāvṛte ati-vego vā na vā niṣ-phala-tāpi vā ।।

śūlaṃ ca pīḍyamāne ca śūlaṃ ca pīḍyamāne tu a 
vā niṣ-phala-tāpi ca
bhukte kukṣau rujā jīrṇe śāmyaty annāvṛte anile ।
mūtrā-pravṛttir ādhmānaṃ vaster mūtrāvṛte bhavet ।।

astau mūtrāvṛte bhavet
viḍ-āvṛte vibandho adhaḥ sva-sthāne parikṛntati ।
vrajaty āśu jarāṃ sneho bhukte cānahyate naraḥ ।।

iḍ-āvṛte ati-viḍ-rodhaḥ 
ve sthāne parikṛntati
śakṛt pīḍitam annena duḥkhaṃ śuṣkaṃ cirāt sṛjet ।
sarva-dhātv-āvṛte vāyau śroṇi-vaṅkṣaṇa-pṛṣṭha-ruk ।।

vilomo māruto a-svasthaṃ hṛdayaṃ pīḍyate ati ca ।
bhramo mūrchā rujā dāhaḥ pittena prāṇa āvṛte ।।

ilomo māruto a-svāsthyaṃ hramo mūrchā rujānāhaḥ
vidagdhe anne ca vamanam udāne api bhramādayaḥ ।
dāho antar ūrjā-bhraṃśaś ca dāho vyāne ca sarva-gaḥ ।।

āho vyāne tu sarva-gaḥ
klamo aṅga-ceṣṭā-saṅgaś ca sa-saṃtāpaḥ sa-vedanaḥ ।
samāna ūṣmopahatir ati-svedo a-ratiḥ sa-tṛṭ ।।

lamo aṅga-ceṣṭā-bhaṅgaś ca
dāhaś ca syād apāne tu male hāridra-varṇa-tā ।
rajo-'tivṛttis tāpaś ca yoni-mehana-pāyuṣu ।।

ajo-'ti-vṛddhis tāpaś ca
śleṣmaṇā tv āvṛte prāṇe sādas tandrā-rucir vamiḥ ।
ṣṭhīvanaṃ kṣavathūdgāra-niḥśvāsocchvāsa-saṃgrahaḥ ।।

udāne guru-gātra-tvam a-rucir vāk-svara-grahaḥ ।
bala-varṇa-praṇāśaś ca vyāne parvāsthi-vāg-grahaḥ ।।

yāne pārśvāsthi-vāg-grahaḥ
guru-tāṅgeṣu sarveṣu skhalitaṃ ca gatau bhṛśam ।
samāne ati-himāṅga-tvam a-svedo manda-vahni-tā ।।

apāne sa-kaphaṃ mūtra-śakṛtaḥ syāt pravartanam ।
iti dvā-viṃśati-vidhaṃ vāyor āvaraṇaṃ viduḥ ।।

pāne sa-kaphaṃ mūtraṃ śakṛtaḥ syāt pravartanam
prāṇādayas tathānyo-'nyam āvṛṇvanti yathā-kramam ।
sarve api viṃśati-vidhaṃ vidyād āvaraṇaṃ ca tat ।।

āvṛṇvanti yathā-yatham
niḥśvāsocchvāsa-saṃrodhaḥ pratiśyāyaḥ śiro-grahaḥ ।
hṛd-rogo mukha-śoṣaś ca prāṇenodāna āvṛte ।।

ṛd-rogo mukha-rogaś ca
udānenāvṛte prāṇe varṇaujo-bala-saṃkṣayaḥ ।
diśānayā ca vibhajet sarvam āvaraṇaṃ bhiṣak ।।

sthānāny avekṣya vātānāṃ vṛddhiṃ hāniṃ ca karmaṇām ।
prāṇādīnāṃ ca pañcānāṃ miśram āvaraṇaṃ mithaḥ ।।

pittādibhir dvā-daśabhir miśrāṇāṃ miśritaiś ca taiḥ ।
miśraiḥ pittādibhis tad-van miśraṇābhir aneka-dhā ।।

tāratamya-vikalpāc ca yāty āvṛtir a-saṃkhya-tām ।
tāṃ lakṣayed avahito yathā-svaṃ lakṣaṇodayāt ।।

śanaiḥ śanaiś copaśayād gūḍhām api muhur muhuḥ ।
viśeṣāj jīvitaṃ prāṇa udāno balam ucyate ।।

syāt tayoḥ pīḍanād dhānir āyuṣaś ca balasya ca ।
āvṛtā vāyavo a-jñātā jñātā vā vatsaraṃ sthitāḥ ।।

prayatnenāpi duḥ-sādhyā bhaveyur vān-upakramāḥ ।
vidradhi-plīha-hṛd-roga-gulmāgni-sadanādayaḥ ।।
bhavanty upadravās teṣām āvṛtānām upekṣaṇāt ।।
vyādhīnāṃ saṃśayaṃ chettum anyato yo a-pramatta-vān ।
nidānaṃ satataṃ tena cintanīyaṃ vipaścitā ।।

cikitsāsthāna
āmāśaya-stho hatvāgniṃ sāmo mārgān pidhāya yat ।
vidadhāti jvaraṃ doṣas tasmāt kurvīta laṅghanam ।।

prāg-rūpeṣu jvarādau vā balaṃ yatnena pālayan ।
balādhiṣṭhānam ārogyam ārogyārthaḥ kriyā-kramaḥ ।।

ārogyārthaṃ kriyā-kramaḥ
laṅghanaiḥ kṣapite doṣe dīpte agnau lāghave sati ।
svāsthyaṃ kṣut tṛḍ ruciḥ paktir balam ojaś ca jāyate ।।

tatrotkṛṣṭe samutkliṣṭe kapha-prāye cale male ।
sa-hṛl-lāsa-prasekānna-dveṣa-kāsa-viṣūcike ।।

sadyo-bhuktasya saṃjāte jvare sāme viśeṣataḥ ।
vamanaṃ vamanārhasya śastaṃ kuryāt tad anya-thā ।।

śvāsātīsāra-saṃmoha-hṛd-roga-viṣama-jvarān ।
pippalībhir yutān gālān kaliṅgair madhukena vā ।।

uṣṇāmbhasā sa-madhunā pibet sa-lavaṇena vā ।
paṭola-nimba-karkoṭa-vetra-pattrodakena vā ।।

tarpaṇena rasenekṣor madyaiḥ kalpoditāni vā ।
vamanāni prayuñjīta bala-kāla-vibhāga-vit ।।

kṛte a-kṛte vā vamane jvarī kuryād viśoṣaṇam ।
doṣāṇāṃ samudīrṇānāṃ pācanāya śamāya ca ।।

doṣeṇa bhasmanevāgnau channe annaṃ na vipacyate ।
tasmād ā-doṣa-pacanāj jvaritān upavāsayet ।।

āmena bhasmanevāgnau
tṛṣṇag alpālpam uṣṇāmbu pibed vāta-kapha-jvare ।
tat kaphaṃ vilayaṃ nītvā tṛṣṇām āśu nivartayet ।।

ṛṣyann alpālpam uṣṇāmbu
udīrya cāgniṃ srotāṃsi mṛdū-kṛtya viśodhayet ।
līna-pittānila-sveda-śakṛn-mūtrānulomanam ।।

nidrā-jāḍyā-ruci-haraṃ prāṇānām avalambanam ।
viparītam ataḥ śītaṃ doṣa-saṃghāta-vardhanam ।।

uṣṇam evaṅ-guṇa-tve api yuñjyān naikānta-pittale ।
udrikta-pitte davathu-dāha-mohātisāriṇi ।।

viṣa-madyotthite grīṣme kṣata-kṣīṇe asra-pittini ।
ghana-candana-śuṇṭhy-ambu-parpaṭośīra-sādhitam ।।

śītaṃ tebhyo hitaṃ toyaṃ pācanaṃ tṛḍ-jvarāpaham ।
ūṣmā pittād ṛte nāsti jvaro nāsty ūṣmaṇā vinā ।।

tasmāt pitta-viruddhāni tyajet pittādhike adhikam ।
snānābhyaṅga-pradehāṃś ca pariśeṣaṃ ca laṅghanam ।।

a-jīrṇa iva śūla-ghnaṃ sāme tīvra-ruji jvare ।
na pibed auṣadhaṃ tad dhi bhūya evāmam āvahet ।।

āmābhibhūta-koṣṭhasya kṣīraṃ viṣam aher iva ।
sodarda-pīnasa-śvāse jaṅghā-parvāsthi-śūlini ।।

aṅghā-pārśvāsthi-śūlini
vāta-śleṣmātmake svedaḥ praśastaḥ sa pravartayet ।
sveda-mūtra-śakṛd-vātān kuryād agneś ca pāṭavam ।।

snehoktam ācāra-vidhiṃ sarva-śaś cānupālayet ।
laṅghanaṃ svedanaṃ kālo yavāgvas tiktako rasaḥ ।।

avāgūs tiktako rasaḥ
malānāṃ pācanāni syur yathāvasthaṃ krameṇa vā ।
śuddha-vāta-kṣayāgantu-jīrṇa-jvariṣu laṅghanam ।।

neṣyate teṣu hi hitaṃ śamanaṃ yan na karśanam ।
tatra sāma-jvarākṛtyā jānīyād a-viśoṣitam ।।

śamanaṃ yan na karṣaṇam
dvi-vidhopakrama-jñānam avekṣeta ca laṅghane ।
yuktaṃ laṅghita-liṅgais tu taṃ peyābhir upācaret ।।

yathā-svauṣadha-siddhābhir maṇḍa-pūrvābhir āditaḥ ।
ṣaḍ-ahaṃ vā mṛdu-tvaṃ vā jvaro yāvad avāpnuyāt ।।

tasyāgnir dīpyate tābhiḥ samidbhir iva pāvakaḥ ।
prāg lāja-peyāṃ su-jarāṃ sa-śuṇṭhī-dhānya-pippalīm ।।

sa-saindhavāṃ tathāmlārthī tāṃ pibet saha-dāḍimām ।
sṛṣṭa-viḍ bahu-pitto vā sa-śuṇṭhī-mākṣikāṃ himām ।।

vasti-pārśva-śiraḥ-śūlī vyāghrī-gokṣura-sādhitām ।
pṛśniparṇī-balā-bilva-nāgarotpala-dhānyakaiḥ ।।

siddhāṃ jvarātisāry amlāṃ peyāṃ dīpana-pācanīm ।
hrasvena pañca-mūlena hikkā-ruk-śvāsa-kāsa-vān ।।

pañca-mūlena mahatā kaphārto yava-sādhitām ।
vibaddha-varcāḥ sa-yavāṃ pippaly-āmalakaiḥ kṛtāṃ ।।

ippaly-āmalakaiḥ śṛtāṃ
yavāgūṃ sarpiṣā bhṛṣṭāṃ mala-doṣānulomanīm ।
cavikā-pippalī-mūla-drākṣāmalaka-nāgaraiḥ ।।

koṣṭhe vibaddhe sa-ruji pibet tu parikartini ।
kola-vṛkṣāmla-kalaśī-dhāvanī-śrīphalaiḥ kṛtām ।।

-dhāvanī-śrī-balā-kṛtām
a-sveda-nidras tṛṣṇārtaḥ sitāmalaka-nāgaraiḥ ।
sitā-badara-mṛdvīkā-śārivā-musta-candanaiḥ ।।

-sveda-nidrā-tṛṣṇārtaḥ
tṛṣṇā-chardi-parīdāha-jvara-ghnīṃ kṣaudra-saṃyutām ।
kuryāt peyauṣadhair eva rasa-yūṣādikān api ।।

ṛṣṇā-chardi-parīvāra- ṛṣṇā-chardi-paro dāha-
madyodbhave madya-nitye pitta-sthāna-gate kaphe ।
grīṣme tayor vādhikayos tṛṭ-chardir-dāha-pīḍite ।।

ṛṭ-chardi-dāha-pīḍite
ūrdhvaṃ pravṛtte rakte ca peyāṃ necchanti teṣu tu ।
jvarāpahaiḥ phala-rasair adbhir vā lāja-tarpaṇāt ।।

dbhir vā lāja-tarpaṇam
pibet sa-śarkarā-kṣaudrān tato jīrṇe tu tarpaṇe ।
yavāgvāṃ vaudanaṃ kṣud-vān aśnīyād bhṛṣṭa-taṇḍulam ।।

ibet sa-śarkarā-kṣaudraṃ ato jīrṇe ca tarpaṇe 
avāgvām odanaṃ kṣud-vān avāgvāṃ caudanaṃ kṣud-vān
daka-lāvaṇikair yūṣai rasair vā mudga-lāva-jaiḥ ।
ity ayaṃ ṣaḍ-aho neyo balaṃ doṣaṃ ca rakṣatā ।।

tataḥ pakveṣu doṣeṣu laṅghanādyaiḥ praśasyate ।
kaṣāyo doṣa-śeṣasya pācanaḥ śamano atha-vā ।।

tiktaḥ pitte viśeṣeṇa prayojyaḥ kaṭukaḥ kaphe ।
pitta-śleṣma-hara-tve api kaṣāyaḥ sa na śasyate ।।

aṣāyas tu na śasyate
nava-jvare mala-stambhāt kaṣāyo viṣama-jvaram ।
kurute a-ruci-hṛl-lāsa-hidhmādhmānādikān api ।।

saptāhād auṣadhaṃ ke-cid āhur anye daśāhataḥ ।
ke-cil laghv-anna-bhuktasya yojyam āmolbaṇe na tu ।।

āhuś cānye daśāhataḥ
tīvra-jvara-parītasya doṣa-vegodaye yataḥ ।
doṣe atha-vāti-nicite tandrā-staimitya-kāriṇi ।।

a-pacyamānaṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ bhūyo jvalayati jvaram ।
mṛdur jvaro laghur dehaś calitāś ca malā yadā ।।

a-cira-jvaritasyāpi bheṣajaṃ yojayet tadā ।
mustayā parpaṭaṃ yuktaṃ śuṇṭhyā duḥsparśayāpi vā ।।

pākyaṃ śīta-kaṣāyaṃ vā pāṭhośīraṃ sa-vālakam ।
pibet tad-vac ca bhūnimba-guḍūcī-musta-nāgaram ।।

yathā-yogam ime yojyāḥ kaṣāyā doṣa-pācanāḥ ।
jvarā-rocaka-tṛṣṇāsya-vairasyā-pakti-nāśanāḥ ।।
kaliṅgakāḥ paṭolasya pattraṃ kaṭuka-rohiṇī ।।
paṭolaṃ śārivā mustā pāṭhā kaṭuka-rohiṇī ।
paṭola-nimba-tri-phalā-mṛdvīkā-musta-vatsakāḥ ।।

kirātatiktam amṛtā candanaṃ viśva-bheṣajam ।
dhātrī-mustāmṛtā-kṣaudram ardha-śloka-samāpanāḥ ।।

pañcaite saṃtatādīnāṃ pañcānāṃ śamanā matāḥ ।
durālabhāmṛtā-mustā-nāgaraṃ vāta-je jvare ।।

atha-vā pippalī-mūla-guḍūcī-viśva-bheṣajam ।
kanīyaḥ pañca-mūlaṃ ca pitte śakrayavā ghanam ।।

itte kṣaudra-samanvitāḥ
kaṭukā ceti sa-kṣaudraṃ mustā-parpaṭakaṃ tathā ।
sa-dhanvayāsa-bhūnimbaṃ vatsakādyo gaṇaḥ kaphe ।।

aliṅga-musta-kaṭukā
atha-vā vṛṣa-gāṅgeyī-śṛṅgavera-durālabhāḥ ।
rug-vibandhānila-śleṣma-yukte dīpana-pācanam ।।

abhayā-pippalī-mūla-śamyāka-kaṭukā-ghanam ।
drākṣā-madhūka-madhuka-lodhra-kāśmarya-śārivāḥ ।।

mustāmalaka-hrīvera-padma-kesara-padmakam ।
mṛṇāla-candanośīra-nīlotpala-parūṣakam ।।

phāṇṭo himo vā drākṣādir jātī-kusuma-vāsitaḥ ।
yukto madhu-sitā-lājair jayaty anila-pitta-jam ।।

jvaraṃ madātyayaṃ chardiṃ mūrchāṃ dāhaṃ śramaṃ bhramam ।
ūrdhva-gaṃ rakta-pittaṃ ca pipāsāṃ kāmalām api ।।

varaṃ madātyayaṃ chardir
pācayet kaṭukāṃ piṣṭvā karpare abhinave śucau ।
niṣpīḍito ghṛta-yutas tad-raso jvara-dāha-jit ।।

kapha-vāte vacā-tiktā-pāṭhāragvadha-vatsakāḥ ।
pippalī-cūrṇa-yukto vā kvāthaś chinnodbhavodbhavaḥ ।।

vyāghrī-śuṇṭhy-amṛtā-kvāthaḥ pippalī-cūrṇa-saṃyutaḥ ।
vāta-śleṣma-jvara-śvāsa-kāsa-pīnasa-śūla-jit ।।

pathyā-kustumburī-mustā-śuṇṭhī-kaṭtṛṇa-parpaṭam ।
sa-kaṭphala-vacā-bhārgī-devāhvaṃ madhu-hiṅgu-mat ।।

kapha-vāta-jvara-ṣṭhīva-kukṣi-hṛt-pārśva-vedanāḥ ।
kaṇṭhāmayāsya-śvayathu-kāsa-śvāsān niyacchati ।।

apha-vāta-jvare ṣṭheva-
āragvadhādiḥ sa-kṣaudraḥ kapha-pitta-jvaraṃ jayet ।
tathā tiktā-vṛṣośīra-trāyantī-tri-phalāmṛtāḥ ।।

paṭolātiviṣā-nimba-mūrvā-dhanvayavāsakāḥ ।
saṃnipāta-jvare vyāghrī-devadāru-niśā-ghanam ।।

paṭola-pattra-nimba-tvak-tri-phalā-kaṭukā-yutam ।
nāgaraṃ pauṣkaraṃ mūlaṃ guḍūcī kaṇṭakārikā ।।

sa-kāsa-śvāsa-pārśvārtau vāta-śleṣmottare jvare ।
madhūka-puṣpa-mṛdvīkā-trāyamāṇā-parūṣakam ।।

sośīra-tiktā-tri-phalā-kāśmaryaṃ kalpayed dhimam ।
kaṣāyaṃ taṃ piban kāle jvarān sarvān apohati ।।

varān sarvān vyapohati
jāty-āmalaka-mustāni tad-vad dhanvayavāsakam ।
baddha-viṭ kaṭukā-drākṣā-trāyantī-tri-phalā-guḍam ।।

-trāyantī-tri-phalā-guḍān -trāyantī-tri-phalā-guḍāḥ
jīrṇauṣadho annaṃ peyādyam ācarec chleṣma-vān na tu ।
peyā kaphaṃ vardhayati paṅkaṃ pāṃsuṣu vṛṣṭi-vat ।।

śleṣmābhiṣyaṇṇa-dehānām ataḥ prāg api yojayet ।
yūṣān kulattha-caṇaka-kalāyādi-kṛtān laghūn ।।

śleṣmābhiṣava-dehānām śleṣmābhispanda-dehānām
rūkṣāṃs tikta-rasopetān hṛdyān ruci-karān paṭūn ।
raktādyāḥ śālayo jīrṇāḥ ṣaṣṭikāś ca jvare hitāḥ ।।

śleṣmottare vīta-tuṣās tathā vāṭī-kṛtā yavāḥ ।
odanas taiḥ sruto dvis triḥ prayoktavyo yathā-yatham ।।

doṣa-dūṣyādi-balato jvara-ghna-kvātha-sādhitaḥ ।
mudgādyair laghubhir yūṣāḥ kulatthaiś ca jvarāpahāḥ ।।

kāravellaka-karkoṭa-bāla-mūlaka-parpaṭaiḥ ।
vārtāka-nimba-kusuma-paṭola-phala-pallavaiḥ ।।

aty-anta-laghubhir māṃsair jāṅgalaiś ca hitā rasāḥ ।
vyāghrī-parūṣa-tarkārī-drākṣāmalaka-dāḍimaiḥ ।।

saṃskṛtāḥ pippalī-śuṇṭhī-dhānya-jīraka-saindhavaiḥ ।
sitā-madhubhyāṃ prāyeṇa saṃyutā vā kṛtā-kṛtāḥ ।।

an-amla-takra-siddhāni rucyāni vyañjanāni ca ।
acchāny anala-saṃpannāny anu-pāne api yojayet ।।

tāni kvathita-śītaṃ ca vāri madyaṃ ca sātmyataḥ ।
sa-jvaraṃ jvara-muktaṃ vā dinānte bhojayel laghu ।।

śleṣma-kṣaya-vivṛddhoṣmā bala-vān analas tadā ।
yathocite atha-vā kāle deśa-sātmyānurodhataḥ ।।

prāg alpa-vahnir bhuñjāno na hy a-jīrṇena pīḍyate ।
kaṣāya-pāna-pathyānnair daśāha iti laṅghite ।।

sarpir dadyāt kaphe mande vāta-pittottare jvare ।
pakveṣu doṣeṣv amṛtaṃ tad viṣopamam anya-thā ।।

daśāhe syād atīte api jvaropadrava-vṛddhi-kṛt ।
laṅghanādi-kramaṃ tatra kuryād ā-kapha-saṃkṣayāt ।।

deha-dhātv-a-bala-tvāc ca jvaro jīrṇo anuvartate ।
rūkṣaṃ hi tejo jvara-kṛt tejasā rūkṣitasya ca ।।

vamana-sveda-kālāmbu-kaṣāya-laghu-bhojanaiḥ ।
yaḥ syād ati-balo dhātuḥ saha-cārī sadā-gatiḥ ।।

tasya saṃśamanaṃ sarpir dīptasyevāmbu veśmanaḥ ।
vāta-pitta-jitām agryaṃ saṃskāraṃ cānurudhyate ।।

aṃskāram anurudhyate
su-tarāṃ tad dhy ato dadyād yathā-svauṣadha-sādhitam ।
viparītaṃ jvaroṣmāṇaṃ jayet pittaṃ ca śaityataḥ ।।

snehād vātaṃ ghṛtaṃ tulyaṃ yoga-saṃskārataḥ kapham ।
pūrve kaṣāyāḥ sa-ghṛtāḥ sarve yojyā yathā-malam ।।

tri-phalā-picumanda-tvaṅ-madhukaṃ bṛhatī-dvayam ।
sa-masūra-dalaṃ kvāthaḥ sa-ghṛto jvara-kāsa-hā ।।

pippalīndrayava-dhāvani-tiktā-śārivāmalaka-tāmalakībhiḥ ।
bilva-musta-hima-pālani-sevyair drākṣayātiviṣayā sthirayā ca ।।

ghṛtam āśu nihanti sādhitaṃ jvaram agniṃ viṣamaṃ halīmakam ।
a-ruciṃ bhṛśa-tāpam aṃsayor vamathuṃ pārśva-śiro-rujaṃ kṣayam ।।

varam ugraṃ viṣamaṃ halīmakam
tailvakaṃ pavana-janmani jvare yojayet trivṛtayā viyojitam ।
tiktakaṃ vṛṣa-ghṛtaṃ ca paittike yac ca pālanikayā śṛtaṃ haviḥ ।।

viḍaṅga-sauvarcala-cavya-pāṭhā-vyoṣāgni-sindhūdbhava-yāva-śūkaiḥ ।
palāṃśakaiḥ kṣīra-samaṃ ghṛtasya prasthaṃ pacej jīrṇa-kapha-jvara-ghnam ।।

alāṃśikaiḥ kṣīra-samaṃ ghṛtasya
guḍūcyā rasa-kalkābhyāṃ tri-phalāyā vṛṣasya vā ।
mṛdvīkāyā balāyāś ca snehāḥ siddhā jvara-cchidaḥ ।।

jīrṇe ghṛte ca bhuñjīta mṛdu-māṃsa-rasaudanam ।
balaṃ hy alaṃ doṣa-haraṃ paraṃ tac ca bala-pradam ।।

ṛdu-māṃsa-rasāśanam
kapha-pitta-harā mudga-kāravellādi-jā rasāḥ ।
prāyeṇa tasmān na hitā jīrṇe vātottare jvare ।।

śūlodāvarta-viṣṭambha-jananā jvara-vardhanāḥ ।
na śāmyaty evam api cej jvaraḥ kurvīta śodhanam ।।

śodhanārhasya vamanaṃ prāg uktaṃ tasya yojayet ।
āmāśaya-gate doṣe balinaḥ pālayan balam ।।

pakve tu śithile doṣe jvare vā viṣa-madya-je ।
modakaṃ tri-phalā-śyāmā-trivṛt-pippali-kesaraiḥ ।।

sa-sitā-madhubhir dadyād vyoṣādyaṃ vā virecanam ।
drākṣā-dhātrī-rasaṃ tad-vat sa-drākṣāṃ vā harītakīm ।।
lihyād vā traivṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ saṃyuktaṃ madhu-sarpiṣā ।।
āragvadhaṃ vā payasā mṛdvīkānāṃ rasena vā ।
tri-phalāṃ trāyamāṇāṃ vā payasā jvaritaḥ pibet ।।

viriktānāṃ ca saṃsargī maṇḍa-pūrvā yathā-kramam ।
cyavamānaṃ jvarotkliṣṭam upekṣeta malaṃ sadā ।।

pakvo api hi vikurvīta doṣaḥ koṣṭhe kṛtāspadaḥ ।
atipravartamānaṃ vā pācayan saṃgrahaṃ nayet ।।

āma-saṃgrahaṇe doṣā doṣopakrama īritāḥ ।
pāyayed doṣa-haraṇaṃ mohād āma-jvare tu yaḥ ।।

āma-saṃgrahaṇād doṣo oṣopakrama īritaḥ
prasuptaṃ kṛṣṇa-sarpaṃ sa karāgreṇa parāmṛśet ।
jvara-kṣīṇasya na hitaṃ vamanaṃ na virecanam ।।

kāmaṃ tu payasā tasya nirūhair vā haren malān ।
kṣīrocitasya prakṣīṇa-śleṣmaṇo dāha-tṛḍ-vataḥ ।।

kṣīraṃ pittānilārtasya pathyam apy atisāriṇaḥ ।
tad vapur laṅghanottaptaṃ pluṣṭaṃ vanam ivāgninā ।।

divyāmbu jīvayet tasya jvaraṃ cāśu niyacchati ।
saṃskṛtaṃ śītam uṣṇaṃ vā tasmād dhāroṣṇam eva vā ।।

ad-vad dhāroṣṇam eva vā
vibhajya kāle yuñjīta jvariṇaṃ hanty ato anya-thā ।
payaḥ sa-śuṇṭhī-kharjūra-mṛdvīkā-śarkarā-ghṛtam ।।

śṛta-śītaṃ madhu-yutaṃ tṛḍ-dāha-jvara-nāśanam ।
tad-vad drākṣā-balā-yaṣṭī-śārivā-kaṇa-candanaiḥ ।।

catur-guṇenāmbhasā vā pippalyā vā śṛtaṃ pibet ।
kāsāc chvāsāc chiraḥ-śūlāt pārśva-śūlāc cira-jvarāt ।।

mucyate jvaritaḥ pītvā pañca-mūlī-śṛtaṃ payaḥ ।
śṛtam eraṇḍa-mūlena bāla-bilvena vā jvarāt ।।

dhāroṣṇaṃ vā payaḥ pītvā vibaddhānila-varcasaḥ ।
sa-rakta-picchātisṛteḥ sa-tṛṭ-śūla-pravāhikāt ।।

siddhaṃ śuṇṭhī-balā-vyāghrī-gokaṇṭaka-guḍaiḥ payaḥ ।
śopha-mūtra-śakṛd-vāta-vibandha-jvara-kāsa-jit ।।

vṛścīva-bilva-varṣābhū-sādhitaṃ jvara-śopha-nut ।
śiṃśipā-sāra-siddhaṃ ca kṣīram āśu jvarāpaham ।।

śiṃśipā-sāra-siddhaṃ vā
nirūhas tu balaṃ vahniṃ vi-jvara-tvaṃ mudaṃ rucim ।
doṣe yuktaḥ karoty āśu pakve pakvāśayaṃ gate ।।

pittaṃ vā kapha-pittaṃ vā pakvāśaya-gataṃ haret ।
sraṃsanaṃ trīn api malān vastiḥ pakvāśayāśrayān ।।

astiḥ pakvāśayāśritān
prakṣīṇa-kapha-pittasya trika-pṛṣṭha-kaṭī-grahe ।
dīptāgner baddha-śakṛtaḥ prayuñjītānuvāsanam ।।

paṭola-nimba-cchadana-kaṭukā-caturaṅgulaiḥ ।
sthirā-balā-gokṣuraka-madanośīra-vālakaiḥ ।।

payasy ardhodake kvāthaṃ kṣīra-śeṣaṃ vimiśritam ।
kalkitair musta-madana-kṛṣṇā-madhuka-vatsakaiḥ ।।

vastiṃ madhu-ghṛtābhyāṃ ca pīḍayej jvara-nāśanam ।
catasraḥ parṇinīr yaṣṭī-phalośīra-nṛpadrumān ।।

kvāthayet kalkayed yaṣṭī-śatāhvā-phalinī-phalam ।
mustaṃ ca vastiḥ sa-guḍa-kṣaudra-sarpir jvarāpahaḥ ।।

jīvantīṃ madanaṃ medāṃ pippalīṃ madhukaṃ vacām ।
ṛddhiṃ rāsnāṃ balāṃ bilvaṃ śatapuṣpāṃ śatāvarīm ।।

piṣṭvā kṣīraṃ jalaṃ sarpis tailaṃ caika-tra sādhitam ।
jvare anuvāsanaṃ dadyād yathā-snehaṃ yathā-malam ।।

vare anuvāsanaṃ dadyāt athā snehaṃ yathā malam 
yathā-doṣaṃ yathā-balam
ye ca siddhiṣu vakṣyante vastayo jvara-nāśanāḥ ।
śiro-rug-gaurava-śleṣma-haram indriya-bodhanam ।।

jīrṇa-jvare ruci-karaṃ dadyān nasyaṃ virecanam ।
snaihikaṃ śūnya-śiraso dāhārte pitta-nāśanam ।।

dhūma-gaṇḍūṣa-kavaḍān yathā-doṣaṃ ca kalpayet ।
pratiśyāyāsya-vairasya-śiraḥ-kaṇṭhāmayāpahān ।।

a-rucau mātuluṅgasya kesaraṃ sājya-saindhavam ।
dhātrī-drākṣā-sitānāṃ vā kalkam āsyena dhārayet ।।

yathopaśaya-saṃsparśān śītoṣṇa-dravya-kalpitān ।
abhyaṅgālepa-sekādīñ jvare jīrṇe tvag-āśrite ।।

kuryād añjana-dhūmāṃś ca tathaivāgantu-je api tān ।
dāhe sahasra-dhautena sarpiṣābhyaṅgam ācaret ।।

sūtroktaiś ca gaṇais tais tair madhurāmla-kaṣāyakaiḥ ।
dūrvādibhir vā pitta-ghnaiḥ śodhanādi-gaṇoditaiḥ ।।

śīta-vīryair hima-sparśaiḥ kvātha-kalkī-kṛtaiḥ pacet ।
tailaṃ sa-kṣīram abhyaṅgāt sadyo dāha-jvaropaham ।।

śiro gātraṃ ca tair eva nāti-piṣṭaiḥ pralepayet ।
tat-kvāthena parīṣekam avagāhaṃ ca yojayet ।।

tathāranāla-salila-kṣīra-śukta-ghṛtādibhiḥ ।
kapittha-mātuluṅgāmla-vidārī-lodhra-dāḍimaiḥ ।।

badarī-pallavotthena phenenāriṣṭakasya vā ।
lipte aṅge dāha-ruṅ-mohāś chardis tṛṣṇā ca śāmyati ।।

henenāriṣṭakasya ca henenāriṣṭa-jena vā
yo varṇitaḥ pitta-haro doṣopakramaṇe kramaḥ ।
taṃ ca śīlayataḥ śīghraṃ sa-dāho naśyati jvaraḥ ।।

vīryoṣṇair uṣṇa-saṃsparśais tagarāguru-kuṅkumaiḥ ।
kuṣṭha-sthauṇeya-śaileya-saralāmaradārubhiḥ ।।

nakha-rāsnā-pura-vacā-caṇḍailā-dvaya-corakaiḥ ।
pṛthvīkā-śigru-surasā-hiṃsrā-dhyāmaka-sarṣapaiḥ ।।

akha-rāsnā-mukha-vacā-
daśa-mūlāmṛtairaṇḍa-dvaya-pattūra-rohiṣaiḥ ।
tamāla-pattra-bhūtīka-śallakī-dhānya-dīpyakaiḥ ।।

amāla-pattra-pūtīka-
miśi-māṣa-kulatthāgni-prakīryā-nākulī-dvayaiḥ ।
anyaiś ca tad-vidhair dravyaiḥ śīte tailaṃ jvare pacet ।।

kvathitaiḥ kalkitair yuktaiḥ surā-sauvīrakādibhiḥ ।
tenābhyañjyāt sukhoṣṇena taiḥ su-piṣṭaiś ca lepayet ।।

enābhyajya sukhoṣṇena
kavoṣṇais taiḥ parīṣekam avagāhaṃ ca kalpayet ।
kevalair api tad-vac ca śukta-go-mūtra-mastubhiḥ ।।

āragvadhādi-vargaṃ ca pānābhyañjana-lepane ।
dhūpān aguru-jān yāṃś ca vakṣyante viṣama-jvare ।।

hūpān aguru-jān ye ca
agny-an-agni-kṛtān svedān svedi bheṣaja-bhojanan ।
garbha-bhū-veśma-śayanaṃ kutha-kambala-rallakān ।।

nir-dhūma-dīptair aṅgārair hasantīś ca hasantikāḥ ।
madyaṃ sa-try-ūṣaṇaṃ takraṃ kulattha-vrīhi-kodravān ।।

saṃśīlayed vepathu-mān yac cānyad api pittalam ।
dayitāḥ stana-śālinyaḥ pīnā vibhrama-bhūṣaṇāḥ ।।

hajec chītārdito yuktyā
yauvanāsava-mattāś ca tam āliṅgeyur aṅganāḥ ।
vīta-śītaṃ ca vijñāya tās tato apanayet punaḥ ।।

īta-śītaṃ tu viyatās
vardhanenaika-doṣasya kṣapaṇenocchritasya vā ।
kapha-sthānānupūrvyā vā tulya-kakṣāñ jayen malān ।।

ṣapaṇenocchritasya ca
śamayet pittam evādau jvareṣu samavāyiṣu ।
dur-nivāra-taraṃ tad dhi jvarārtānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
chardi-mūrchā-pipāsādīn a-virodhāñ jvarasya tu ।।
saṃnipāta-jvarasyānte karṇa-mūle su-dāruṇaḥ ।
śophaḥ saṃjāyate yena kaś-cid eva vimucyate ।।

śophaḥ saṃjāyate tena aś-cid eva pramucyate
raktāvasecanaiḥ śīghraṃ sarpiḥ-pānaiś ca taṃ jayet ।
pradehaiḥ kapha-pitta-ghnair nāvanaiḥ kavaḍa-grahaiḥ ।।

radehaiḥ kapha-vāta-ghnair
śītoṣṇa-snigdha-rūkṣādyair jvaro yasya na śāmyati ।
śākhānusārī tasyāśu muñced bāhvoḥ kramāt sirām ।।

ayam eva vidhiḥ kāryo viṣame api yathā-yatham ।
jvare vibhajya vātādīn yaś cān-antaram ucyate ।।

iṣame ca yathā-yatham
paṭola-kaṭukā-mustā-prāṇadā-madhukaiḥ kṛtāḥ ।
tri-catuḥ-pañca-śaḥ kvāthā viṣama-jvara-nāśanāḥ ।।

yojayet tri-phalāṃ pathyāṃ guḍūcīṃ pippalīṃ pṛthak ।
tais tair vidhānaiḥ sa-guḍaṃ bhallātakam athāpi vā ।।

laṅghanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ vādau jvarāgamana-vāsare ।
prātaḥ sa-tailaṃ laśunaṃ prāg-bhaktaṃ vā tathā ghṛtam ।।

aṅghanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ vāpi
jīrṇaṃ tad-vad dadhi payas takraṃ sarpiś ca ṣaṭ-palam ।
kalyāṇakaṃ pañca-gavyaṃ tiktākhyaṃ vṛṣa-sādhitam ।।

tri-phalā-kola-tarkārī-kvāthe dadhnā śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।
tilvaka-tvak-kṛtāvāpaṃ viṣama-jvara-jit param ।।

surāṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca yan madyaṃ śikhi-tittiri-dakṣa-jam ।
māṃsaṃ medyoṣṇa-vīryaṃ ca sahānnena pra-kāmataḥ ।।

śikhi-tittiri-kukkuṭāt āṃsaṃ madhyoṣṇa-vīryaṃ ca 
āṃsaṃ medhyoṣṇa-vīryaṃ ca
sevitvā tad-ahaḥ svapyād atha-vā punar ullikhet ।
sarpiṣo mahatīṃ mātrāṃ pītvā vā chardayet punaḥ ।।

nīlinīm ajagandhāṃ ca trivṛtāṃ kaṭu-rohiṇīm ।
pibej jvarasyāgamane sneha-svedopapāditaḥ ।।

manohvā saindhavaṃ kṛṣṇā tailena nayanāñjanam ।
yojyaṃ hiṅgu-samā vyāghrī-vasā nasyaṃ sa-saindhavam ।।

purāṇa-sarpiḥ siṃhasya vasā tad-vat sa-saindhavā ।
palaṅkaṣā nimba-pattraṃ vacā kuṣṭhaṃ harītakī ।।

sarṣapāḥ sa-yavāḥ sarpir dhūpo viḍ vā biḍāla-jā ।
pura-dhyāma-vacā-sarja-nimbārkāguru-dārubhiḥ ।।

dhūpo jvareṣu sarveṣu kāryo ayam a-parājitaḥ ।
dhūpa-nasyāñjanottrāsā ye coktāś citta-vaikṛte ।।

rayoktavyo a-parājitaḥ hūpa-nasyāñjana-trāsā
daivāśrayaṃ ca bhaiṣajyaṃ jvarān sarvān vyapohati ।
viśeṣād viṣamān prāyas te hy āgantv-anubandha-jāḥ ।।

yathā-svaṃ ca sirāṃ vidhyed a-śāntau viṣama-jvare ।
kevalānila-vīsarpa-visphoṭābhihata-jvare ।।

-śānte viṣama-jvare -visphoṭābhihate jvare
sarpiḥ-pāna-himālepa-seka-māṃsa-rasāśanam ।
kuryād yathā-svam uktaṃ ca rakta-mokṣādi sādhanam ।।

arpiḥ-pānaṃ himālepa- -sekān māṃsa-rasāśanam
grahotthe bhūta-vidyoktaṃ bali-mantrādi sādhanam ।
oṣadhi-gandha-je pitta-śamanaṃ viṣa-jid viṣe ।।

uṣadhi-gandha-je pitta-
iṣṭair arthair mano-jñaiś ca yathā-doṣa-śamena ca ।
hitā-hita-vivekaiś ca jvaraṃ krodhādi-jaṃ jayet ।।

krodha-jo yāti kāmena śāntiṃ krodhena kāma-jaḥ ।
bhaya-śokodbhavau tābhyāṃ bhī-śokābhyāṃ tathetarau ।।

śāpātharvaṇa-mantrotthe vidhir daiva-vyapāśrayaḥ ।
te jvarāḥ kevalāḥ pūrvaṃ vyāpyante an-antaram malaiḥ ।।

tasmād doṣānusāreṇa teṣv āhārādi kalpayet ।
na hi jvaro anubadhnāti mārutādyair vinā kṛtaḥ ।।

jvara-kāla-smṛtiṃ cāsya hāribhir viṣayair haret ।
karuṇārdraṃ manaḥ śuddhaṃ sarva-jvara-vināśanam ।।

arva-jvara-vimokṣaṇam
tyajed ā-bala-lābhāc ca vyāyāma-snāna-maithunam ।
gurv-a-sātmya-vidāhy annaṃ yac cānyaj jvara-kāraṇam ।।

na vi-jvaro api sahasā sarvānnīno bhavet tathā ।
nivṛtto api jvaraḥ śīghraṃ vyāpādayati dur-balam ।।

arvānnīno bhavet tadā ivṛtto hi jvaraḥ śīghraṃ
sadyaḥ prāṇa-haro yasmāt tasmāt tasya viśeṣataḥ ।
tasyāṃ tasyām avasthāyāṃ tat tat kuryād bhiṣag-jitam ।।

at tat kuryāc cikitsitam
oṣadhayo maṇayaś ca su-mantrāḥ sādhu-guru-dvi-ja-daivata-pūjāḥ ।
prīti-karā manaso viṣayāś ca ghnanty api viṣṇu-kṛtaṃ jvaram ugram ।।

uṣadhayo maṇayaś ca su-mantrāḥ

cikitsāsthāna
ūrdhva-gaṃ balino a-vegam eka-doṣānugaṃ navam ।
rakta-pittaṃ sukhe kāle sādhayen nir-upadravam ।।

adho-gaṃ yāpayed raktaṃ yac ca doṣa-dvayānugam ।
śāntaṃ śāntaṃ punaḥ kupyan mārgān mārgāntaraṃ ca yat ।।

ati-pravṛttaṃ mandāgnes tri-doṣaṃ dvi-pathaṃ tyajet ।
jñātvā nidānam ayanaṃ malāv anu-balau balam ।।

deśa-kālādy-avasthāṃ ca rakta-pitte prayojayet ।
laṅghanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ vādau śodhanaṃ śamanaṃ tathā ।।

aṅghanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ cādau
saṃtarpaṇotthaṃ balino bahu-doṣasya sādhayet ।
ūrdhva-bhāgaṃ virekeṇa vamanena tv adho-gatam ।।

amanena tv adho-gamam
śamanair bṛṃhaṇaiś cānyal laṅghya-bṛṃhyān avekṣya ca ।
ūrdhvaṃ pravṛtte śamanau rasau tikta-kaṣāyakau ।।

aṅghya-bṛṃhyān apekṣya ca
upavāsaś ca niḥ-śuṇṭhī-ṣaḍ-aṅgodaka-pāyinaḥ ।
adho-ge rakta-pitte tu bṛṃhaṇo madhuro rasaḥ ।।

ūrdhva-ge tarpaṇaṃ yojyaṃ prāk ca peyā tv adho-gate ।
aśnato balino a-śuddhaṃ na dhāryaṃ tad dhi roga-kṛt ।।

eyā pūrvam adho-gate rāk ca peyā tv adho-game ā prāk 
peyā tv adho-game
dhārayed anya-thā śīghram agni-vac chīghra-kāri tat ।
trivṛc-chyāmā-kaṣāyeṇa kalkena ca sa-śarkaram ।।

gala-grahaṃ pūti-nasyaṃ mūrchāyam a-ruciṃ jvaram ।
gulmaṃ plīhānam ānāhaṃ kilāsaṃ mūtra-kṛcchra-tām ।।

kuṣṭhāny arśāṃsi vīsarpaṃ varṇa-nāśaṃ bhagandaram ।
buddhīndriyoparodhaṃ ca kuryāt stambhitam āditaḥ ।।

sādhayed vidhi-val lehaṃ lihyāt pāṇi-talaṃ tataḥ ।
trivṛtā tri-phalā śyāmā pippalī śarkarā madhu ।।

modakaḥ saṃnipātordhva-rakta-śopha-jvarāpahaḥ ।
trivṛt sama-sitā tad-vat pippalī-pāda-saṃyutā ।।

-rakta-pitta-jvarāpahaḥ
vamanaṃ phala-saṃyuktaṃ tarpaṇaṃ sa-sitā-madhu ।
sa-sitaṃ vā jalaṃ kṣaudra-yuktaṃ vā madhukodakam ।।

kṣīraṃ vā rasam ikṣor vā śuddhasyān-antaro vidhiḥ ।
yathā-svaṃ mantha-peyādiḥ prayojyo rakṣatā balam ।।

mantho jvarokto drākṣādiḥ pitta-ghnair vā phalaiḥ kṛtaḥ ।
madhu-kharjūra-mṛdvīkā-parūṣaka-sitāmbhasā ।।

mantho vā pañca-sāreṇa sa-ghṛtair lāja-saktubhiḥ ।
dāḍimāmalakāmlo vā mandāgny-amlābhilāṣiṇām ।।

andāgny-amlābhilāṣiṇaḥ
kamalotpala-kiñjalka-pṛśniparṇī-priyaṅgukāḥ ।
uśīraṃ śabaraṃ lodhraṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ ku-candanam ।।

hrīveraṃ dhātakī-puṣpaṃ bilva-madhyaṃ durālabhā ।
ardhārdhair vihitāḥ peyā vakṣyante pāda-yaugikāḥ ।।

rdharcair vihitāḥ peyā rdhārdha-vihitāḥ peyā
bhūnimba-sevya-jaladā masūrāḥ pṛśniparṇy api ।
vidārigandhā mudgāś ca balā sarpir hareṇukāḥ ।।

alā sarpiḥ priyaṅgukāḥ
jāṅgalāni ca māṃsāni śīta-vīryāṇi sādhayet ।
pṛthak pṛthag jale teṣāṃ yavāgūḥ kalpayed rase ।।

śītāḥ sa-śarkarā-kṣaudrās tad-van māṃsa-rasān api ।
īṣad-amlān an-amlān vā ghṛta-bhṛṣṭān sa-śarkarān ।।

śūka-śimbī-bhavaṃ dhānyaṃ rakte śākaṃ ca śasyate ।
anna-sva-rūpa-vijñāne yad uktaṃ laghu-śītalam ।।

pūrvoktam ambu pānīyaṃ pañca-mūlena vā śṛtam ।
laghunā śṛta-śītaṃ vā madhv-ambho vā phalāmbu vā ।।

śaśaḥ sa-vāstukaḥ śasto vibandhe tittiriḥ punaḥ ।
udumbarasya niryūhe sādhito mārute adhike ।।

plakṣasya barhiṇas tad-van nyagrodhasya ca kukkuṭaḥ ।
yat kiñ-cid rakta-pittasya nidānaṃ tac ca varjayet ।।

vāsā-rasena phalinī-mṛl-lodhrāñjana-mākṣikam ।
pittāsṛk śamayet pītaṃ niryāso vāṭarūṣakāt ।।

śarkarā-madhu-saṃyuktaḥ kevalo vā śṛto api vā ।
vṛṣaḥ sadyo jayaty asraṃ sa hy asya param auṣadham ।।

paṭola-mālatī-nimba-candana-dvaya-padmakam ।
lodhro vṛṣas taṇḍulīyaḥ kṛṣṇā mṛn madayantikā ।।

aṭolāmalakī-nimba-
śatāvarī gopakanyā kākolyau madhuyaṣṭikā ।
rakta-pitta-harāḥ kvāthās trayaḥ sa-madhu-śarkarāḥ ।।

palāśa-valka-kvātho vā su-śītaḥ śarkarānvitaḥ ।
lihyād vā madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ gavāśva-śakṛto rasam ।।

ibed vā madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ
sa-kṣaudraṃ grathite rakte lihyāt pārāvatāc chakṛt ।
ati-niḥsruta-raktaś ca kṣaudreṇa rudhiraṃ pibet ।।

ihyāt pārāvataṃ śakṛt ti-niḥsṛta-raktaś ca 
ti-niḥsṛta-rakto vā ti-niḥsruta-rakto vā
jāṅgalaṃ bhakṣayed vājam āmaṃ pitta-yutaṃ yakṛt ।
candanośīra-jalada-lāja-mudga-kaṇā-yavaiḥ ।।

balā-jale paryuṣitaiḥ kaṣāyo rakta-pitta-hā ।
prasādaś candanāmbho-ja-sevya-mṛd-bhṛṣṭa-loṣṭa-jaḥ ।।

su-śītaḥ sa-sitā-kṣaudraḥ śoṇitāti-pravṛtti-jit ।
āpothya vā nave kumbhe plāvayed ikṣu-gaṇḍikāḥ ।।

sthitaṃ tad guptam ākāśe rātriṃ prātaḥ srutaṃ jalam ।
madhu-mad vikacāmbho-ja-kṛtottaṃsaṃ ca tad-guṇam ।।

ye ca pitta-jvare coktāḥ kaṣāyās tāṃś ca yojayet ।
kaṣāyair vividhair ebhir dīpte agnau vijite kaphe ।।

rakta-pittaṃ na cec chāmyet tatra vātolbaṇe payaḥ ।
yuñjyāc chāgaṃ śṛtaṃ tad-vad gavyaṃ pañca-guṇe ambhasi ।।

pañca-mūlena laghunā śṛtaṃ vā sa-sitā-madhu ।
jīvakarṣabhaka-drākṣā-balā-gokṣura-nāgaraiḥ ।।

pṛthak pṛthak śṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ sa-ghṛtaṃ sitayātha-vā ।
gokaṇṭakābhīru-śṛtaṃ parṇinībhis tathā payaḥ ।।

hanty āśu raktaṃ sa-rujaṃ viśeṣān mūtra-mārga-gam ।
viṇ-mārga-ge viśeṣeṇa hitaṃ moca-rasena tu ।।

vaṭa-prarohair śuṅgair vā śuṇṭhy-udīcyotpalair api ।
raktātīsāra-dur-nāma-cikitsāṃ cātra kalpayet ।।

aṭa-prarohair śṛṅgair vā
pītvā kaṣāyān payasā bhuñjīta payasaiva ca ।
kaṣāya-yogair ebhir vā vipakvaṃ pāyayed ghṛtam ।।

sa-mūla-mastakaṃ kṣuṇṇaṃ vṛṣam aṣṭa-guṇe ambhasi ।
paktvāṣṭāṃśāvaśeṣeṇa ghṛtaṃ tena vipācayet ।।

tat-puṣpa-garbhaṃ tac chītaṃ sa-kṣaudraṃ pitta-śoṇitam ।
pitta-gulma-jvara-śvāsa-kāsa-hṛd-roga-kāmalāḥ ।।

timira-bhrama-vīsarpa-svara-sādāṃś ca nāśayet ।
palāśa-vṛnta-sva-rase tad-garbhaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ pacet ।।

sa-kṣaudraṃ tac ca rakta-ghnaṃ tathaiva trāyamāṇayā ।
rakte sa-picche sa-kaphe grathite kaṇṭha-mārga-ge ।।

lihyān mākṣika-sarpirbhyāṃ kṣāram utpala-nāla-jam ।
pṛthak pṛthak tathāmbho-ja-reṇu-śyāmā-madhūka-jam ।।

gudāgame viśeṣeṇa śoṇite vastir iṣyate ।
ghrāṇa-ge rudhire śuddhe nāvanaṃ cānuṣecayet ।।

kaṣāya-yogān pūrvoktān kṣīrekṣv-ādi-rasāplutān ।
kṣīrādīn sa-sitāṃs toyaṃ kevalaṃ vā jalaṃ hitaṃ ।।

ṣīrekṣv-ādi-rasa-plutān
raso dāḍima-puṣpāṇām āmrāsthnaḥ śādvalasya vā ।
kalpayec chīta-vargaṃ ca pradehābhyañjanādiṣu ।।

āmrāsthnaḥ śādvalasya ca
su-sūkṣmā māṣa-piṣṭī ca ghṛta-bhṛṣṭā śivasya ca ।
ruṇaddhi mūrdha-lepena nāsā-raktaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।

yac ca pitta-jvare proktaṃ bahir antaś ca bheṣajam ।
rakta-pitte hitaṃ tac ca kṣata-kṣīṇe hitaṃ ca yat ।।

cikitsāsthāna
kevalānila-jaṃ kāsaṃ snehair ādāv upācaret ।
vāta-ghna-siddhaiḥ snigdhaiś ca peyā-yūṣa-rasādibhiḥ ।।

lehair dhūmais tathābhyaṅga-sveda-sekāvagāhanaiḥ ।
vastibhir baddha-viḍ-vātaṃ sa-pittaṃ tūrdhva-bhaktikaiḥ ।।

a-pittaṃ vordhva-bhaktikaiḥ a-pittaṃ vordhva-bhaktikaiḥ
ghṛtaiḥ kṣīraiś ca sa-kaphaṃ jayet sneha-virecanaiḥ ।
guḍūcī-kaṇṭakārībhyāṃ pṛthak triṃśat-palād rase ।।

prasthaḥ siddho ghṛtād vāta-kāsa-nud vahni-dīpanaḥ ।
kṣāra-rāsnā-vacā-hiṅgu-pāṭhā-yaṣṭy-āhva-dhānyakaiḥ ।।

dvi-śāṇaiḥ sarpiṣaḥ prasthaṃ pañca-kola-yutaiḥ pacet ।
daśa-mūlasya niryūhe pīto maṇḍānupāyinā ।।

sa kāsa-śvāsa-hṛt-pārśva-grahaṇī-roga-gulma-nut ।
droṇe apāṃ sādhayed rāsnā-daśa-mūla-śatāvarīḥ ।।

palonmitā dvi-kuḍavaṃ kulatthaṃ badaraṃ yavaṃ ।
tulārdhaṃ cāja-māṃsasya tena sādhyaṃ ghṛtāḍhakam ।।

sama-kṣīraṃ palāṃśaiś ca jīvanīyaiḥ samīkṣya tat ।
prayuktaṃ vāta-rogeṣu pāna-nāvana-vastibhiḥ ।।

pañca-kāsāñ chiraḥ-kampaṃ yoni-vaṅkṣaṇa-vedanām ।
sarvāṅgaikāṅga-rogāṃś ca sa-plīhordhvānilāñ jayet ।।

vidāry-ādi-gaṇa-kvātha-kalka-siddhaṃ ca kāsa-jit ।
aśoka-bīja-kṣavaka-jantughnāñjana-padmakaiḥ ।।

sa-viḍaiś ca ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ tac-cūrṇaṃ vā ghṛta-plutam ।
lihyāt payaś cānupibed ājaṃ kāsāti-pīḍitaḥ ।।

ājaṃ kāsābhipīḍitaḥ ājaṃ kāsādi-pīḍitaḥ
viḍaṅgaṃ nāgaraṃ rāsnā pippalī hiṅgu saindhavam ।
bhārgī kṣāraś ca tac cūrṇaṃ pibed vā ghṛta-mātrayā ।।

sa-kaphe anila-je kāse śvāsa-hidhmā-hatāgniṣu ।
durālabhāṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ śaṭhīṃ drākṣāṃ sitopalām ।।

śuṇṭhīṃ drākṣāṃ sitopalām
lihyāt karkaṭaśṛṅgīṃ ca kāse tailena vāta-je ।
duḥsparśāṃ pippalīṃ mustāṃ bhārgīṃ karkaṭakīṃ śaṭhīm ।।

purāṇa-guḍa-tailābhyāṃ cūrṇitāny avalehayet ।
tad-vat sa-kṛṣṇāṃ śuṇṭhīṃ ca sa-bhārgīṃ tad-vad eva ca ।।

pibec ca kṛṣṇāṃ koṣṇena salilena sa-saindhavām ।
mastunā sa-sitāṃ śuṇṭhīṃ dadhnā vā kaṇa-reṇukām ।।

adhnā vā kaṇa-reṇukam
pibed badara-majjño vā madirā-dadhi-mastubhiḥ ।
atha-vā pippalī-kalkaṃ ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaṃ sa-saindhavam ।।

ibed badara-majjāṃ vā
kāsī sa-pīnaso dhūmaṃ snaihikaṃ vidhinā pibet ।
hidhmā-śvāsokta-dhūmāṃś ca kṣīra-māṃsa-rasāśanaḥ ।।

grāmyānūpaudakaiḥ śāli-yava-godhūma-ṣaṣṭikān ।
rasair māṣātmaguptānāṃ yūṣair vā bhojayed dhitān ।।

rāmyānūpodbhavaiḥ śāli-
yavānī-pippalī-bilva-madhya-nāgara-citrakaiḥ ।
rāsnājājī-pṛthakparṇī-palāśa-śaṭhi-pauṣkaraiḥ ।।

siddhāṃ snigdhāmla-lavaṇāṃ peyām anila-je pibet ।
kaṭī-hṛt-pārśva-koṣṭhārti-śvāsa-hidhmā-praṇāśanīm ।।

daśa-mūla-rase tad-vat pañca-kola-guḍānvitām ।
pibet peyāṃ sama-tilāṃ kṣaireyīṃ vā sa-saindhavām ।।

mātsya-kaukkuṭa-vārāhair māṃsair vā sājya-saindhavām ।
vāstuko vāyasī-śākaṃ kāsaghnaḥ suniṣaṇṇakaḥ ।।

kaṇṭakāryāḥ phalaṃ pattraṃ bālaṃ śuṣkaṃ ca mūlakam ।
snehās tailādayo bhakṣyāḥ kṣīrekṣu-rasa-gauḍikāḥ ।।

dadhi-mastv-āranālāmla-phalāmbu-madirāḥ pibet ।
pitta-kāse tu sa-kaphe vamanaṃ sarpiṣā hitam ।।

tathā madana-kāśmarya-madhuka-kvathitair jalaiḥ ।
phala-yaṣṭy-āhva-kalkair vā vidārīkṣu-rasāplutaiḥ ।।

pitta-kāse tanu-kaphe trivṛtāṃ madhurair yutām ।
yuñjyād virekāya yutāṃ ghana-śleṣmaṇi tiktakaiḥ ।।

hṛta-doṣo himaṃ svādu snigdhaṃ saṃsarjanaṃ bhajet ।
ghane kaphe tu śiśiraṃ rūkṣaṃ tiktopasaṃhitam ।।

lehaḥ paitte sitā-dhātrī-kṣaudra-drākṣā-himotpalaiḥ ।
sa-ghṛtaḥ sānile hitaḥ sa-kaphe sābda-maricaḥ ।।

ehaḥ pitte sitā-dhātrī-
mṛdvīkārdha-śataṃ triṃśat pippalīḥ śarkarā-palam ।
lehayen madhunā gor vā kṣīra-pasya śakṛd-rasam ।।

tvag-elā-vyoṣa-mṛdvīkā-pippalī-mūla-pauṣkaraiḥ ।
lāja-mustā-śaṭhī-rāsnā-dhātrī-phala-vibhītakaiḥ ।।

śarkarā-kṣaudra-sarpirbhir leho hṛd-roga-kāsa-hā ।
madhurair jāṅgala-rasair yava-śyāmāka-kodravāḥ ।।

mudgādi-yūṣaiḥ śākaiś ca tiktakair mātrayā hitāḥ ।
ghana-śleṣmaṇi lehāś ca tiktakā madhu-saṃyutāḥ ।।

śālayaḥ syus tanu-kaphe ṣaṣṭikāś ca rasādibhiḥ ।
śarkarāmbho anu-pānārthaṃ drākṣekṣu-sva-rasāḥ payaḥ ।।

kākolī-bṛhatī-medā-dvayaiḥ sa-vṛṣa-nāgaraiḥ ।
pitta-kāse rasa-kṣīra-peyā-yūṣān prakalpayet ।।

drākṣāṃ kaṇāṃ pañca-mūlaṃ tṛṇākhyaṃ ca pacej jale ।
tena kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ śītaṃ pibet sa-madhu-śarkaram ।।

sādhitāṃ tena peyāṃ vā su-śītāṃ madhunānvitām ।
śaṭhī-hrīvera-bṛhatī-śarkarā-viśva-bheṣajam ।।

piṣṭvā rasaṃ pibet pūtaṃ vastreṇa ghṛta-mūrchitam ।
medāṃ vidārīṃ kākolīṃ svayaṅguptā-phalaṃ balām ।।

śarkarāṃ jīvakaṃ mudga-māṣaparṇyau durālabhām ।
kalkī-kṛtya pacet sarpiḥ kṣīreṇāṣṭa-guṇena tat ।।

pāna-bhojana-leheṣu prayuktaṃ pitta-kāsa-jit ।
lihyād vā cūrṇam eteṣāṃ kaṣāyam atha-vā pibet ।।

kapha-kāsī pibed ādau surakāṣṭhāt pradīpitāt ।
snehaṃ parisrutaṃ vyoṣa-yava-kṣārāvacūrṇitam ।।

apha-kāse pibed ādau
snigdhaṃ virecayed ūrdhvam adho mūrdhni ca yuktitaḥ ।
tīkṣṇair virekair balinaṃ saṃsargīṃ cāsya yojayet ।।

yava-mudga-kulatthānnair uṣṇa-rūkṣaiḥ kaṭūtkaṭaiḥ ।
kāsamardaka-vārtāka-vyāghrī-kṣāra-kaṇānvitaiḥ ।।

dhānva-baila-rasaiḥ snehais tila-sarṣapa-nimba-jaiḥ ।
daśa-mūlāmbu gharmāmbu madyaṃ madhv-ambu vā pibet ।।

hānva-baila-rasair lehais ila-sarṣapa-bilva-jaiḥ
mūlaiḥ pauṣkara-śamyāka-paṭolaiḥ saṃsthitaṃ niśām ।
pibed vāri saha-kṣaudraṃ kāleṣv annasya vā triṣu ।।

-paṭolair anvitaṃ niśām
pippalī pippalī-mūlaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ vibhītakam ।
śikhi-kukkuṭa-picchānāṃ maṣī kṣāro yavodbhavaḥ ।।

viśālā pippalī-mūlaṃ trivṛtā ca madhu-dravāḥ ।
kapha-kāsa-harā lehās trayaḥ ślokārdha-yojitāḥ ।।

madhunā maricaṃ lihyān madhunaiva ca joṅgakam ।
pṛthag rasāṃś ca madhunā vyāghrī-vārtāka-bhṛṅga-jān ।।

kāsaghnasyāśva-śakṛtaḥ surasasyāsitasya ca ।
devadāru-śaṭhī-rāsnā-karkaṭākhyā-durālabhāḥ ।।

urasasyāsitasya vā
pippalī nāgaraṃ mustaṃ pathyā dhātrī sitopalā ।
lājāḥ sitopalā sarpiḥ śṛṅgī dhātrī-phalodbhavā ।।

śṛṅgī dhātrī-phalād rajaḥ
madhu-taila-yutā lehās trayo vātānuge kaphe ।
dve pale dāḍimād aṣṭau guḍād vyoṣāt pala-trayam ।।

rocanaṃ dīpanaṃ svaryaṃ pīnasa-śvāsa-kāsa-jit ।
guḍa-kṣāroṣaṇa-kaṇā-dāḍimaṃ śvāsa-kāsa-jit ।।

-dāḍimāc chvāsa-kāsa-jit
kramāt pala-dvayārdhākṣa-karṣārdhākṣa-palonmitam ।
pibej jvaroktaṃ pathyādi sa-śṛṅgīkaṃ ca pācanam ।।

-karṣākṣārdha-palonmitam
atha-vā dīpyaka-trivṛd-viśālā-ghana-pauṣkaram ।
sa-kaṇaṃ kvathitaṃ mūtre kapha-kāsī jale api vā ।।

taila-bhṛṣṭaṃ ca vaidehī-kalkākṣaṃ sa-sitopalam ।
pāyayet kapha-kāsa-ghnaṃ kulattha-salilāplutam ।।

daśa-mūlāḍhake prasthaṃ ghṛtasyākṣa-samaiḥ pacet ।
puṣkarāhva-śaṭhī-bilva-surasā-vyoṣa-hiṅgubhiḥ ।।

uṣkarākhya-śaṭhī-bilva-
peyānu-pānaṃ tat sarva-vāta-śleṣmāmayāpaham ।
nirguṇḍī-pattra-niryāsa-sādhitaṃ kāsa-jid ghṛtam ।।
ghṛtaṃ rase viḍaṅgānāṃ vyoṣa-garbhaṃ ca sādhitam ।।punarnava-śivātikā-sarala-kāsamardāmṛtā- ।।paṭola-bṛhatī-phaṇijjaka-rasaiḥ payaḥ-saṃyutaiḥ ।।ghṛtaṃ tri-kaṭunā ca siddham upayujya saṃjāyate ।।na kāsa-viṣama-jvara-kṣaya-gudāṅkurebhyo bhayam ।।sa-mūla-phala-pattrāyāḥ kaṇṭakāryā rasāḍhake ।।
a-mūla-phala-śākhāyāḥ
ghṛta-prasthaṃ balā-vyoṣa-viḍaṅga-śaṭhi-dāḍimaiḥ ।
sauvarcala-yava-kṣāra-mūlāmalaka-pauṣkaraiḥ ।।

vṛścīva-bṛhatī-pathyā-yavānī-citrakarddhibhiḥ ।
mṛdvīkā-cavya-varṣābhū-durālabhāmla-vetasaiḥ ।।

śṛṅgī-tāmalakī-bhārgī-rāsnā-gokṣurakaiḥ pacet ।
kalkais tat sarva-kāseṣu śvāsa-hidhmāsu ceṣyate ।।

kaṇṭakārī-ghṛtaṃ caitat kapha-vyādhi-vināśanam ।
paced vyāghrī-tulāṃ kṣuṇṇāṃ vahe apām āḍhaka-sthite ।।

kṣipet pūte tu saṃcūrṇya vyoṣa-rāsnāmṛtāgnikān ।
śṛṅgī-bhārgī-ghana-granthi-dhanvayāsān palārdhakān ।।

ṣipet pūte ca saṃcūrṇya
sarpiṣaḥ ṣo-ḍaśa-palaṃ catvāriṃśat palāni ca ।
matsyaṇḍikāyāḥ śuddhāyāḥ punaś ca tad adhiśrayet ।।

darvī-lepini śīte ca pṛthag dvi-kuḍavaṃ kṣipet ।
pippalīnāṃ tavakṣīryā mākṣikasyā-navasya ca ।।

ippalīnāṃ tukākṣīryā
leho ayaṃ gulma-hṛd-roga-dur-nāma-śvāsa-kāsa-jit ।
śamanaṃ ca pibed dhūmaṃ śodhanaṃ bahale kaphe ।।

śodhanaṃ bahule kaphe
manaḥśilāla-madhuka-māṃsī-musteṅgudī-tvacaḥ ।
dhūmaṃ kāsa-ghna-vidhinā pītvā kṣīraṃ pibed anu ।।

niṣṭhyūtānte guḍa-yutaṃ koṣṇaṃ dhūmo nihanti saḥ ।
vāta-śleṣmottarān kāsān a-cireṇa ciran-tanān ।।

tamakaḥ kapha-kāse tu syāc cet pittānubandha-jaḥ ।
pitta-kāsa-kriyāṃ tatra yathāvasthaṃ prayojayet ।।

kaphānubandhe pavane kuryāt kapha-harāṃ kriyām ।
pittānubandhayor vāta-kaphayoḥ pitta-nāśinīm ।।

vāta-śleṣmātmake śuṣke snigdham ārdre virūkṣaṇam ।
kāse karma sa-pitte tu kapha-je tikta-saṃyutam ।।

nigdhaṃ cārdre virūkṣaṇam
urasy antaḥ-kṣate sadyo lākṣāṃ kṣaudra-yutāṃ pibet ।
kṣīreṇa śālīn jīrṇe adyāt kṣīreṇaiva sa-śarkarān ।।

pārśva-vasti-sa-ruk cālpa-pittāgnis tāṃ surā-yutām ।
bhinna-viṭkaḥ sa-mustātiviṣā-pāṭhāṃ sa-vatsakām ।।

lākṣāṃ sarpir madhūcchiṣṭaṃ jīvanīyaṃ gaṇaṃ sitām ।
tvakkṣīrīṃ samitaṃ kṣīre paktvā dīptānalaḥ pibet ।।

vakkṣīrīṃ saṃmitaṃ kṣīre
ikṣvārikā-bisa-granthi-padma-kesara-candanaiḥ ।
śṛtaṃ payo madhu-yutaṃ saṃdhānārthaṃ pibet kṣatī ।।

yavānāṃ cūrṇam āmānāṃ kṣīre siddhaṃ ghṛtānvitam ।
jvara-dāhe sitā-kṣaudra-saktūn vā payasā pibet ।।

ṣīra-siddhaṃ ghṛtānvitam
kāsa-vāṃs tu pibet sarpir madhurauṣadha-sādhitam ।
guḍodakaṃ vā kvathitaṃ sa-kṣaudra-maricaṃ hitam ।।

āsa-vāṃś ca pibet sarpir
cūrṇam āmalakānāṃ vā kṣīre pakvaṃ ghṛtānvitam ।
rasāyana-vidhānena pippalīr vā prayojayet ।।

ṣīra-pakvaṃ ghṛtānvitam
kāsī parvāsthi-śūlī ca lihyāt sa-ghṛta-mākṣikāḥ ।
madhūka-madhuka-drākṣā-tvakkṣīrī-pippalī-balāḥ ।।

ihyāt sa-ghṛta-mākṣikān -tvakkṣīrī-pippalī-balān
tri-jātam ardha-karṣāṃśaṃ pippaly-ardha-palaṃ sitā ।
drākṣā madhūkaṃ kharjūraṃ palāśaṃ ślakṣṇa-cūrṇitam ।।

madhunā guṭikā ghnanti tā vṛṣyāḥ pitta-śoṇitam ।
kāsa-śvāsā-ruci-cchardi-mūrchā-hidhmā-mada-bhramān ।।

-mūrchā-hidhmā-vami-bhramān
kṣata-kṣaya-svara-bhraṃśa-plīha-śoṣāḍhya-mārutān ।
rakta-niṣṭhīva-hṛt-pārśva-ruk-pipāsā-jvarān api ।।

-plīha-śophāḍhya-mārutān
varṣābhū-śarkarā-rakta-śāli-taṇḍula-jaṃ rajaḥ ।
rakta-ṣṭhīvī pibet siddhaṃ drākṣā-rasa-payo-ghṛtaiḥ ।।

madhūka-madhuka-kṣīra-siddhaṃ vā taṇḍulīyakam ।
yathā-svaṃ mārga-visṛte rakte kuryāc ca bheṣajam ।।

mūḍha-vātas tv ajā-medaḥ surā-bhṛṣṭaṃ sa-saindhavam ।
kṣāmaḥ kṣīṇaḥ kṣatorasko manda-nidro agni-dīpti-mān ।।

śṛta-kṣīra-sareṇādyāt sa-ghṛta-kṣaudra-śarkaram ।
śarkarā-yava-godhūmaṃ jīvakarṣabhakau madhu ।।

śarkarāṃ yava-godhūmaṃ
śṛta-kṣīrānu-pānaṃ vā lihyāt kṣīṇaḥ kṣataḥ kṛśaḥ ।
kravyāt-piśita-niryūhaṃ ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaṃ pibec ca saḥ ।।

pippalī-kṣaudra-saṃyuktaṃ māṃsa-śoṇita-vardhanam ।
nyagrodhodumbarāśvattha-plakṣa-śāla-priyaṅgubhiḥ ।।

tāla-mastaka-jambū-tvak-priyālaiś ca sa-padmakaiḥ ।
sāśvakarṇaiḥ śṛtāt kṣīrād adyāj jātena sarpiṣā ।।

śāly-odanaṃ kṣatoraskaḥ kṣīṇa-śukra-balendriyaḥ ।
vāta-pittārdite abhyaṅgo gātra-bhede ghṛtair mataḥ ।।

tailaiś cānila-roga-ghnaiḥ pīḍite mātariśvanā ।
hṛt-pārśvārtiṣu pānaṃ syāj jīvanīyasya sarpiṣaḥ ।।

ṛta-pārśvārtau tu pānaṃ syāj
kuryād vā vāta-roga-ghnaṃ pitta-raktā-virodhi yat ।
yaṣṭy-āhva-nāgabalayoḥ kvāthe kṣīra-same ghṛtam ।।

payasyā-pippalī-vāṃśī-kalkaiḥ siddhaṃ kṣate hitam ।
jīvanīyo gaṇaḥ śuṇṭhī varī vīrā punarnavā ।।

balā-bhārgī-svaguptarddhi-śaṭhī-tāmalakī-kaṇāḥ ।
śṛṅgāṭakaṃ payasyā ca pañca-mūlaṃ ca yal laghu ।।

drākṣākṣoṭādi ca phalaṃ madhura-snigdha-bṛṃhaṇam ।
taiḥ pacet sarpiṣaḥ prasthaṃ karṣāṃśaiḥ ślakṣṇa-kalkitaiḥ ।।

kṣīra-dhātrī-vidārīkṣu-cchāga-māṃsa-rasānvitam ।
prasthārdhaṃ madhunaḥ śīte śarkarārdha-tulā-rajaḥ ।।

palārdhakaṃ ca marica-tvag-elā-pattra-kesaram ।
vinīya prasṛtaṃ tasmāl lihyān mātrāṃ yathā-balam ।।

ihyān mātrāṃ yathānalam
amṛta-prāśam ity etan narāṇām amṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।
sudhāmṛta-rasaṃ prāśyaṃ kṣīra-māṃsa-rasāśinā ।।

naṣṭa-śukra-kṣata-kṣīṇa-dur-bala-vyādhi-karśitān ।
strī-prasaktān kṛśān varṇa-svara-hīnāṃś ca bṛṃhayet ।।

-dur-bala-vyādhi-karṣitān
kāsa-hidhmā-jvara-śvāsa-dāha-tṛṣṇāsra-pitta-nut ।
putra-daṃ chardi-mūrchā-hṛd-yoni-mūtrāmayāpaham ।।

śvadaṃṣṭrośīra-mañjiṣṭhā-balā-kāśmarya-kaṭtṛṇam ।
darbha-mūlaṃ pṛthakparṇīṃ palāśarṣabhakau sthirām ।।

pālikāni pacet teṣāṃ rase kṣīra-catur-guṇe ।
kalkaiḥ svaguptā-jīvantī-medarṣabhaka-jīvakaiḥ ।।

śatāvary-ṛddhi-mṛdvīkā-śarkarā-śrāvaṇī-bisaiḥ ।
prasthaḥ siddho ghṛtād vāta-pitta-hṛd-roga-śūla-nut ।।

-pitta-hṛd-drava-śūla-nut
mūtra-kṛcchra-pramehārśaḥ-kāsa-śoṣa-kṣayāpahaḥ ।
dhanuḥ-strī-madya-bhārādhva-khinnānāṃ bala-māṃsa-daḥ ।।

madhukāṣṭa-pala-drākṣā-prastha-kvāthe paced ghṛtam ।
pippaly-aṣṭa-pale kalke prasthaṃ siddhe ca śītale ।।

pṛthag aṣṭa-palaṃ kṣaudra-śarkarābhyāṃ vimiśrayet ।
sama-saktu kṣata-kṣīṇa-rakta-gulmeṣu tad dhitam ।।

dhātrī-phala-vidārīkṣu-jīvanīya-rasād ghṛtāt ।
gavyājayoś ca payasoḥ prasthaṃ prasthaṃ vipācayet ।।

siddha-śīte sitā-kṣaudraṃ dvi-prasthaṃ vinayet tataḥ ।
yakṣmāpasmāra-pittāsṛk-kāsa-meha-kṣayāpaham ।।

iddha-pūte sitā-kṣaudraṃ -kāsa-meha-jvarāpaham
vayaḥ-sthāpanam āyuṣyaṃ māṃsa-śukra-bala-pradam ।
ghṛtaṃ tu pitte abhyadhike lihyād vāte adhike pibet ।।

ihyād vātādhike pibet
līḍhaṃ nirvāpayet pittam alpa-tvād dhanti nānalam ।
ākrāmaty anilaṃ pītam ūṣmāṇaṃ niruṇaddhi ca ।।

kṣāma-kṣīṇa-kṛśāṅgānām etāny eva ghṛtāni tu ।
tvakkṣīrī-śarkarā-lāja-cūrṇaiḥ styānāni yojayet ।।

vakkṣīrī-pippalī-lāja- -cūrṇaiḥ pānāni yojayet
sarpir-guḍān sa-madhv-aṃśān kṛtvā dadyāt payo anu ca ।
reto vīryaṃ balaṃ puṣṭiṃ tair āśu-taram āpnuyāt ।।

vīta-tvag-asthi-kūṣmāṇḍa-tulāṃ svinnāṃ punaḥ pacet ।
ghaṭṭayan sarpiṣaḥ prasthe kṣaudra-varṇe atra ca kṣipet ।।

ṣaudra-varṇe tu nikṣipet
khaṇḍāc chataṃ kaṇā-śuṇṭhyor dvi-palaṃ jīrakād api ।
tri-jāta-dhānya-maricaṃ pṛthag ardha-palāṃśakam ।।

avatārita-śīte ca dattvā kṣaudraṃ ghṛtārdhakam ।
khajenāmathya ca sthāpyaṃ tan nihanty upayojitam ।।

kāsa-hidhmā-jvara-śvāsa-rakta-pitta-kṣata-kṣayān ।
uraḥ-saṃdhāna-jananaṃ medhā-smṛti-bala-pradam ।।

aśvibhyāṃ vihitaṃ hṛdyaṃ kūṣmāṇḍaka-rasāyanam ।
piben nāgabalā-mūlasyārdha-karṣābhivardhitam ।।

ṃyārdha-karṣādi-vardhitam ṃyārdha-karṣa-vivardhitam
palaṃ kṣīra-yutaṃ māsaṃ kṣīra-vṛttir an-anna-bhuk ।
eṣa prayogaḥ puṣṭy-āyur-bala-varṇa-karaḥ param ।।

maṇḍūkaparṇyāḥ kalpo ayaṃ yaṣṭyā viśvauṣadhasya ca ।
pāda-śeṣaṃ jala-droṇe pacen nāgabalā-tulām ।।

tena kvāthena tulyāṃśaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ ca sādhayet ।
palārdhikaiś cātibalā-balā-yaṣṭī-punarnavaiḥ ।।

prapauṇḍarīka-kāśmarya-priyāla-kapikacchubhiḥ ।
aśvagandhā-sitābhīru-medā-yugma-trikaṇṭakaiḥ ।।

kākolī-kṣīra-kākolī-kṣīraśuklā-dvi-jīrakaiḥ ।
mṛṇāla-bisa-kharjūra-śṛṅgāṭaka-kaserukaiḥ ।।

-kṣīraśuklā-dvi-jīvakaiḥ
etan nāgabalā-sarpiḥ pitta-rakta-kṣata-kṣayān ।
jayet tṛḍ-bhrama-dāhāṃś ca bala-puṣṭi-karaṃ param ।।

varṇyam āyuṣyam ojasyaṃ valī-palita-nāśanam ।
upayujya ca ṣaṇ māsān vṛddho api taruṇāyate ।।

payujya tu ṣaṇ-māsād
dīpte agnau vidhir eṣa syān mande dīpana-pācanaḥ ।
yakṣmoktaḥ kṣatināṃ śasto grāhī śakṛti tu drave ।।

daśa-mūlaṃ svayaṅguptāṃ śaṅkhapuṣpīṃ śaṭhīṃ balām ।
hasti-pippaly-apāmārga-pippalī-mūla-citrakān ।।

bhārgīṃ puṣkara-mūlaṃ ca dvi-palāṃśaṃ yavāḍhakam ।
harītakī-śataṃ caikaṃ jala-pañcāḍhake pacet ।।

vi-palāṃśān yavāḍhakam ale pañcāḍhake pacet
yava-svede kaṣāyaṃ taṃ pūtaṃ tac cābhayā-śatam ।
paced guḍa-tulāṃ dattvā kuḍavaṃ ca pṛthag ghṛtāt ।।

ave svinne kaṣāyaṃ taṃ
tailāt sa-pippalī-cūrṇāt siddha-śīte ca mākṣikāt ।
lehaṃ dve cābhaye nityam ataḥ khāded rasāyanāt ।।

ehe dve cābhaye nityam
tad valī-palitaṃ hanyād varṇāyur-bala-vardhanam ।
pañca-kāsān kṣayaṃ śvāsaṃ sa-hidhmaṃ viṣama-jvaram ।।

meha-gulma-grahaṇy-arśo-hṛd-rogā-ruci-pīnasān ।
agastya-vihitaṃ dhanyam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rasāyanam ।।

daśa-mūlaṃ balāṃ mūrvāṃ haridre pippalī-dvayam ।
pāṭhāśvagandhāpāmārga-svaguptātiviṣāmṛtāḥ ।।

aridrā-pippalī-dvayam -svaguptātiviṣāmṛtam
bāla-bilvaṃ trivṛd-dantī-mūlaṃ pattraṃ ca citrakāt ।
payasyāṃ kuṭajaṃ hiṃsrāṃ puṣpaṃ sāraṃ ca bījakāt ।।

boṭa-sthavira-bhallāta-vikaṅkata-śatāvarīḥ ।
pūti-karañja-śamyāka-candralekhā-sahācaram ।।

-candralekhā-sahācarāt
śaubhāñjanaka-nimba-tvag-ikṣuraṃ ca palāṃśakam ।
pathyā-sahasraṃ sa-śataṃ yavānāṃ cāḍhaka-dvayam ।।

paced aṣṭa-guṇe toye yava-svede avatārayet ।
pūte kṣipet sa-pathye ca tatra jīrṇa-guḍāt tulām ।।

ūte kṣipet sa-pathyāṃ ca
tailājya-dhātrī-rasataḥ prasthaṃ prasthaṃ tataḥ punaḥ ।
adhiśrayen mṛdāv agnau darvī-lepe avatārya ca ।।

śīte prastha-dvayaṃ kṣaudrāt pippalī-kuḍavaṃ kṣipet ।
cūrṇī-kṛtaṃ tri-jātāc ca tri-palaṃ nikhanet tataḥ ।।

dhānye purāṇa-kumbha-sthaṃ māsaṃ khādec ca pūrva-vat ।
rasāyanaṃ vasiṣṭhoktam etat pūrva-guṇādhikam ।।

svasthānāṃ niṣ-parīhāraṃ sarvartuṣu ca śasyate ।
pālikaṃ saindhavaṃ śuṇṭhī dve ca sauvarcalāt pale ।।

kuḍavāṃśāni vṛkṣāmlaṃ dāḍimaṃ pattram ārjakāt ।
ekaikāṃ maricājājyor dhānyakād dve caturthike ।।

āḍimaṃ pattram ārjakam
śarkarāyāḥ palāny atra daśa dve ca pradāpayet ।
kṛtvā cūrṇam ato mātrām anna-pāneṣu dāpayet ।।

rucyaṃ tad dīpanaṃ balyaṃ pārśvārti-śvāsa-kāsa-jit ।
ekāṃ ṣo-ḍaśikāṃ dhānyād dve dve cājāji-dīpyakāt ।।

ārśvārti-śvāsa-kāsa-nut
tābhyāṃ dāḍima-vṛkṣāmle dvir dviḥ sauvarcalāt palam ।
śuṇṭhyāḥ karṣaṃ dadhitthasya madhyāt pañca palāni ca ।।

śuṇṭhyāḥ karṣaṃ kapitthasya
tac cūrṇaṃ ṣo-ḍaśa-palaiḥ śarkarāyā vimiśrayet ।
ṣāḍavo ayaṃ pradeyaḥ syād anna-pāneṣu pūrva-vat ।।

vidhiś ca yakṣma-vihito yathāvasthaṃ kṣate hitaḥ ।
nivṛtte kṣata-doṣe tu kaphe vṛddha uraḥ śiraḥ ।।

dālyate kāsino yasya sa nā dhūmān pibed imān ।
dvi-medā-dvi-balā-yaṣṭī-kalkaiḥ kṣaume su-bhāvite ।।

ālyete kāsino yasya a dhūmān nā pibed imān
vartiṃ kṛtvā pibed dhūmaṃ jīvanīya-ghṛtānupaḥ ।
manaḥśilā-palāśājagandhā-tvakkṣīri-nāgaraiḥ ।।

tad-vad evānu-pānaṃ tu śarkarekṣu-guḍodakam ।
piṣṭvā manaḥśilāṃ tulyām ārdrayā vaṭa-śuṅgayā ।।

sa-sarpiṣkaṃ pibed dhūmaṃ tittiri-pratibhojanam ।
kṣaya-je bṛṃhaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ kuryād agneś ca vardhanam ।।

ittiri-pratibhojitam
bahu-doṣāya sa-snehaṃ mṛdu dadyād virecanam ।
śamyākena trivṛtayā mṛdvīkā-rasa-yuktayā ।।

tilvakasya kaṣāyeṇa vidārī-sva-rasena ca ।
sarpiḥ siddhaṃ pibed yuktyā kṣīṇa-deho viśodhanam ।।

pitte kaphe dhātuṣu ca kṣīṇeṣu kṣaya-kāsa-vān ।
ghṛtaṃ karkaṭakī-kṣīra-dvi-balā-sādhitaṃ pibet ।।

vidārībhiḥ kadambair vā tāla-sasyaiś ca sādhitam ।
ghṛtaṃ payaś ca mūtrasya vaivarṇye kṛcchra-nirgame ।।

śūne sa-vedane meḍhre pāyau sa-śroṇi-vaṅkṣaṇe ।
ghṛta-maṇḍena laghunānuvāsyo miśrakeṇa vā ।।

jāṅgalair pratibhuktasya vartakādyā bile-śayāḥ ।
krama-śaḥ prasahās tad-vat prayojyāḥ piśitāśinaḥ ।।

auṣṇyāt pramāthi-bhāvāc ca srotobhyaś cyāvayanti te ।
kaphaṃ śuddhaiś ca taiḥ puṣṭiṃ kuryāt samyag vahan rasaḥ ।।

cavikā-tri-phalā-bhārgī-daśa-mūlaiḥ sa-citrakaiḥ ।
kulattha-pippalī-mūla-pāṭhā-kola-yavair jale ।।

śṛtair nāgara-duḥsparśā-pippalī-śaṭhi-pauṣkaraiḥ ।
piṣṭaiḥ karkaṭaśṛṅgyā ca samaiḥ sarpir vipācayet ।।

siddhe asmiṃś cūrṇitau kṣārau dvau pañca lavaṇāni ca ।
dattvā yuktyā piben mātrāṃ kṣaya-kāsa-nipīḍitaḥ ।।

vau pañca lavaṇāni tu
kāsamardābhayā-mustā-pāṭhā-kaṭphala-nāgaraiḥ ।
pippalyā kaṭu-rohiṇyā kāśmaryā surasena ca ।।

akṣa-mātrair ghṛta-prasthaṃ kṣīra-drākṣā-rasāḍhake ।
pacec choṣa-jvara-plīha-sarva-kāsa-haraṃ śivam ।।

vṛṣa-vyāghrī-guḍūcīnāṃ pattra-mūla-phalāṅkurāt ।
rasa-kalkair ghṛtaṃ pakvaṃ hanti kāsa-jvarā-rucīḥ ।।

dvi-guṇe dāḍima-rase siddhaṃ vā vyoṣa-saṃyutam ।
pibed upari bhuktasya yava-kṣāra-yutaṃ naraḥ ।।

ibed upari bhaktasya ava-kṣāra-ghṛtaṃ naraḥ 
yava-kṣāra-yutaṃ ghṛtam
pippalī-guḍa-siddhaṃ vā chāga-kṣīra-yutaṃ ghṛtam ।
etāny agni-vivṛddhy-arthaṃ sarpīṃṣi kṣaya-kāsinām ।।

syur doṣa-baddha-kaṇṭhoraḥ-srotasāṃ ca viśuddhaye ।
prasthonmite yava-kvāthe viṃśatiṃ vijayāḥ pacet ।।

svinnā mṛditvā tās tasmin purāṇāt ṣaṭ-palaṃ guḍāt ।
pippalyā dvi-palaṃ karṣaṃ manohvāyā rasāñjanāt ।।

dattvārdhākṣaṃ paced bhūyaḥ sa lehaḥ śvāsa-kāsa-jit ।
śvāvidhāṃ sūcayo dagdhāḥ sa-ghṛta-kṣaudra-śarkarāḥ ।।

a lehaḥ śvāsa-kāsa-nut
śvāsa-kāsa-harā barhi-pādau vā madhu-sarpiṣā ।
eraṇḍa-pattra-kṣāraṃ vā vyoṣa-taila-guḍānvitam ।।

lehayet kṣāram evaṃ vā surasairaṇḍa-pattra-jam ।
lihyāt try-ūṣaṇa-cūrṇaṃ vā purāṇa-guḍa-sarpiṣā ।।

padmakaṃ tri-phalā vyoṣaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ devadāru ca ।
balā rāsnā ca tac-cūrṇaṃ samastaṃ sama-śarkaram ।।

amasta-sama-śarkaram
khāden madhu-ghṛtābhyāṃ vā lihyāt kāsa-haraṃ param ।
tad-van marica-cūrṇaṃ vā sa-ghṛta-kṣaudra-śarkaram ।।

ad-van marica-cūrṇaṃ ca
pathyā-śuṇṭhī-ghana-guḍair guṭikāṃ dhārayen mukhe ।
sarveṣu śvāsa-kāseṣu kevalaṃ vā vibhītakam ।।

pattra-kalkaṃ ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaṃ tilvakasya sa-śarkaram ।
peyā votkārikā chardi-tṛṭ-kāsāmātisāra-jit ।।

eyā cotkārikā chardi- -tṛṭ-kāsāmātisāra-nut
kaṇṭakārī-rase siddho kṣīraṃ yūṣān rasān api ।
sa-gaurāmalakaḥ sāmlaḥ sarva-kāsa-bhiṣag-jitam ।।

vāta-ghnauṣadha-niḥkvāthe kṣīraṃ yūṣān rasān api ।
vaiṣkirān prātudān bailān dāpayet kṣaya-kāsine ।।

kṣata-kāse ca ye dhūmāḥ sānu-pānā nidarśitāḥ ।
kṣaya-kāse api te yojyā vakṣyate yac ca yakṣmaṇi ।।

akṣyante ye ca yakṣmaṇi
bṛṃhaṇaṃ dīpanaṃ cāgneḥ srotasāṃ ca viśodhanam ।
vyatyāsāt kṣaya-kāsibhyo balyaṃ sarvaṃ praśasyate ।।

saṃnipātodbhavo ghoraḥ kṣaya-kāso yatas tataḥ ।
yathā-doṣa-balaṃ tasya saṃnipāta-hitaṃ hitam ।।

cikitsāsthāna
śvāsa-hidhmā yatas tulya-hetv-ādyāḥ sādhanaṃ tataḥ ।
tulyam eva tad-ārtaṃ ca pūrvaṃ svedair upācaret ।।

snigdhair lavaṇa-tailāktaṃ taiḥ kheṣu grathitaḥ kaphaḥ ।
su-līno api vilīno asya koṣṭhaṃ prāptaḥ su-nirharaḥ ।।

srotasāṃ syān mṛdu-tvaṃ ca marutaś cānuloma-tā ।
svinnaṃ ca bhojayed annaṃ snigdham ānūpa-jai rasaiḥ ।।

ārutasyānuloma-tā
dadhy-uttareṇa vā dadyāt tato asmai vamanaṃ mṛdu ।
viśeṣāt kāsa-vamathu-hṛd-graha-svara-sādine ।।

pippalī-saindhava-kṣaudra-yuktaṃ vātā-virodhi yat ।
nirhṛte sukham āpnoti sa kaphe duṣṭa-vigrahe ।।

srotaḥsu ca viśuddheṣu caraty a-vihato anilaḥ ।
dhmānodāvarta-tamake mātuluṅgāmla-vetasaiḥ ।।

hiṅgu-pīlu-viḍair yuktam annaṃ syād anulomanam ।
sa-saindhavaṃ phalāmlaṃ vā koṣṇaṃ dadyād virecanam ।।

ete hi kapha-saṃruddha-gati-prāṇa-prakopa-jāḥ ।
tasmāt tan-mārga-śuddhy-artham ūrdhvādhaḥ śodhanaṃ hitam ।।

udīryate bhṛśa-taraṃ mārga-rodhād vahaj jalam ।
yathā tathānilas tasya mārgam asmād viśodhayet ।।

a-śāntau kṛta-saṃśuddher dhūmair līnaṃ malaṃ haret ।
haridrā-pattram eraṇḍa-mūlaṃ lākṣāṃ manaḥśilām ।।

-mūlaṃ drākṣāṃ manaḥśilām
sa-devadārv alaṃ māṃsīṃ piṣṭvā vartiṃ prakalpayet ।
tāṃ ghṛtāktāṃ pibed dhūmaṃ yavān vā ghṛta-saṃyutān ।।

madhūcchiṣṭaṃ sarja-rasaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā guru vāguru ।
candanaṃ vā tathā śṛṅgaṃ vālān vā snāva vā gavām ।।

ālān vā snāyu vā gavām
ṛkṣa-godhā-kuraṅgaiṇa-carma-śṛṅga-khurāṇi vā ।
gugguluṃ vā manohvāṃ vā śāla-niryāsam eva vā ।।

ṛśya-godhā-kuraṅgaiṇa- -carma-śṛṅga-khurāṇi ca
śallakīṃ gugguluṃ lohaṃ padmakaṃ vā ghṛtāplutam ।
avaśyaṃ svedanīyānām a-svedyānām api kṣaṇam ।।

admakaṃ vā ghṛta-plutam
svedayet sa-sitā-kṣīra-sukhoṣṇa-sneha-secanaiḥ ।
utkārikopanāhaiś ca svedādhyāyokta-bheṣajaiḥ ।।

uraḥ kaṇṭhaṃ ca mṛdubhiḥ sāme tv āma-vidhiṃ caret ।
ati-yogoddhataṃ vātaṃ dṛṣṭvā pavana-nāśanaiḥ ।।

snigdhai rasādyair nāty-uṣṇair abhyaṅgaiś ca śamaṃ nayet ।
an-utkliṣṭa-kaphā-svinna-dur-balānāṃ hi śodhanāt ।।

vāyur labdhāspado marma saṃśoṣyāśu hared asūn ।
kaṣāya-leha-snehādyais teṣāṃ saṃśamayed ataḥ ।।

kṣīṇa-kṣatātisārāsṛk-pitta-dāhānubandha-jān ।
madhura-snigdha-śītādyair hidhmā-śvāsān upācaret ।।

kulattha-daśa-mūlānāṃ kvāthe syur jāṅgalā rasāḥ ।
yūṣāś ca śigru-vārtāka-kāsaghna-vṛṣa-mūlakaiḥ ।।

pallavair nimba-kulaka-bṛhatī-mātuluṅga-jaiḥ ।
vyāghrī-durālabhā-śṛṅgī-bilva-madhya-trikaṇṭakaiḥ ।।

sāmṛtāgni-kulatthaiś ca yūṣaḥ syāt kvathitair jale ।
tad-vad rāsnā-bṛhaty-ādi-balā-mudgaiḥ sa-citrakaiḥ ।।

ūṣaḥ syāt kvathitair jalaiḥ
peyā ca citrakājājī-śṛṅgī-sauvarcalaiḥ kṛtā ।
daśa-mūlena vā kāsa-śvāsa-hidhmā-rujāpahā ।।

daśa-mūla-śaṭhī-rāsnā-bhārgī-bilvarddhi-pauṣkaraiḥ ।
kulīraśṛṅgī-capalā-tāmalaky-amṛtauṣadhaiḥ ।।

pibet kaṣāyaṃ jīrṇe asmin peyāṃ tair eva sādhitām ।
śāli-ṣaṣṭika-godhūma-yava-mudga-kulattha-bhuk ।।

kāsa-hṛd-graha-pārśvārti-hidhmā-śvāsa-praśāntaye ।
saktūn vārkāṅkura-kṣīra-bhāvitānāṃ sa-mākṣikān ।।

yavānāṃ daśa-mūlādi-niḥkvātha-lulitān pibet ।
anne ca yojayet kṣāra-hiṅgv-ājya-viḍa-dāḍimān ।।

sa-pauṣkara-śaṭhī-vyoṣa-mātuluṅgāmla-vetasān ।
daśa-mūlasya vā kvātham atha-vā devadāruṇaḥ ।।

aśa-mūlasya niḥkvātham
pibed vā vāruṇī-maṇḍaṃ hidhmā-śvāsī pipāsitaḥ ।
pippalī-pippalī-mūla-pathyā-jantughna-citrakaiḥ ।।

kalkitair lepite rūḍhe niḥkṣiped ghṛta-bhājane ।
takraṃ māsa-sthitaṃ tad dhi dīpanaṃ śvāsa-kāsa-jit ।।

pāṭhāṃ madhurasāṃ dāru saralaṃ ca niśi sthitam ।
surā-maṇḍe alpa-lavaṇaṃ pibet prasṛta-saṃmitam ।।

aralaṃ niśi saṃsthitam ibet prasṛti-saṃmitam
bhārgī-śuṇṭhyau sukhāmbhobhiḥ kṣāraṃ vā maricānvitam ।
sva-kvātha-piṣṭāṃ lulitāṃ bāṣpikāṃ pāyayeta vā ।।

sva-rasaḥ saptaparṇasya puṣpāṇāṃ vā śirīṣataḥ ।
hidhmā-śvāse madhu-kaṇā-yuktaḥ pitta-kaphānuge ।।

utkārikā tugā-kṛṣṇā-madhūlī-ghṛta-nāgaraiḥ ।
pittānubandhe yoktavyā pavane tv anubandhini ।।

śvāvic-chaśāmiṣa-kaṇā-ghṛta-śalyaka-śoṇitaiḥ ।
suvarcalā-rasa-vyoṣa-sarpirbhiḥ sahitaṃ payaḥ ।।

anu śāly-odanaṃ peyam vāta-pittānubandhini ।
catur-guṇāmbu-siddhaṃ vā chāgaṃ sa-guḍa-nāgaram ।।

pippalī-mūla-madhuka-guḍa-go-'śva-śakṛd-rasān ।
hidhmābhiṣyanda-kāsa-ghnāō̃ lihyān madhu-ghṛtānvitān ।।

go-gajāśva-varāhoṣṭra-khara-meṣāja-viḍ-rasam ।
sa-madhv ekaika-śo lihyād bahu-śleṣmātha-vā pibet ।।

catuṣ-pāc-carma-romāsthi-khura-śṛṅgodbhavāṃ maṣīm ।
tathaiva vājigandhāyā lihyāc chvāsī kapholbaṇaḥ ।।

śaṭhī-pauṣkara-dhātrīr vā pauṣkaraṃ vā kaṇānvitam ।
gairikāñjana-kṛṣṇā vā sva-rasaṃ vā kapittha-jam ।।

rasena vā kapitthasya dhātrī-saindhava-pippalīḥ ।
ghṛta-kṣaudreṇa vā pathyā-viḍaṅgoṣaṇa-pippalīḥ ।।

kola-lājāmala-drākṣā-pippalī-nāgarāṇi vā ।
guḍa-taila-niśā-drākṣā-kaṇā-rāsnoṣaṇāni vā ।।

pibed rasāmbu-madyāmlair lehauṣadha-rajāṃsi vā ।
jīvantī-musta-surasa-tvag-elā-dvaya-pauṣkaram ।।

caṇḍā-tāmalakī-loha-bhārgī-nāgara-vālakam ।
karkaṭākhyā-śaṭhī-kṛṣṇā-nāgakesara-corakam ।।

upayuktaṃ yathā-kāmaṃ cūrṇaṃ dvi-guṇa-śarkaram ।
pārśva-rug-jvara-kāsa-ghnaṃ hidhmā-śvāsa-haraṃ param ।।

śaṭhī-tāmalakī-bhārgī-caṇḍā-vālaka-pauṣkaram ।
śarkarāṣṭa-guṇaṃ cūrṇaṃ hidhmā-śvāsa-haraṃ param ।।

tulyaṃ guḍaṃ nāgaraṃ ca bhakṣayen nāvayeta vā ।
laśunasya palāṇḍor vā mūlaṃ gṛñjanakasya vā ।।

candanād vā rasaṃ dadyān nārī-kṣīreṇa nāvanam ।
stanyena makṣikā-viṣṭhām alaktaka-rasena vā ।।

sa-saindhavaṃ ghṛtācchaṃ vā siddhaṃ stanyena vā ghṛtam ।
kalkitair madhura-dravyais tat piben nāvayeta vā ।।

sakṛd uṣṇaṃ sakṛc chītaṃ vyatyāsāt sa-sitā-madhu ।
tad-vat payas tathā siddham adho-bhāgauṣadhair ghṛtam ।।

kaṇā-sauvarcala-kṣāra-vayaḥsthā-hiṅgu-corakaiḥ ।
sa-kāyasthair ghṛtaṃ mastu-daśa-mūla-rase pacet ।।

tat pibej jīvanīyair vā lihyāt sa-madhu sādhitam ।
tejovaty abhayā kuṣṭhaṃ pippalī kaṭu-rohiṇī ।।

bhūtikaṃ pauṣkaraṃ mūlaṃ palāśaś citrakaḥ śaṭhī ।
paṭu-dvayaṃ tāmalakī jīvantī bilva-peśikā ।।

vacā pattraṃ ca tālīśaṃ karṣāṃśais tair vipācayet ।
hiṅgu-pādair ghṛta-prasthaṃ pītam āśu nihanti tat ।।

acā pattraṃ ca tālīśāt
śākhānilārśo-grahaṇī-hidhmā-hṛt-pārśva-vedanāḥ ।
ardhāṃśena pibet sarpiḥ kṣāreṇa paṭunātha-vā ।।

dhānvantaraṃ vṛṣa-ghṛtaṃ dādhikaṃ hapuṣādi vā ।
śītāmbu-sekaḥ sahasā trāsa-vikṣepa-bhī-śucaḥ ।।

harṣerṣyocchvāsa-rodhāś ca hitaṃ kīṭaiś ca daṃśanam ।
yat kiñ-cit kapha-vāta-ghnam uṣṇaṃ vātānulomanam ।।

arṣerṣyocchvāsa-saṃrodhā
tat sevyaṃ prāya-śo yac ca su-tarāṃ mārutāpaham ।
sarveṣāṃ bṛṃhaṇe hy alpaḥ śakyaś ca prāya-śo bhavet ।।

nāty-arthaṃ śamane apāyo bhṛśo a-śakyaś ca karṣaṇe ।
śamanair bṛṃhaṇaiś cāto bhūyiṣṭhaṃ tān upācaret ।।

hṛśo a-śakyaś ca karśane kāsa-śvāsa-kṣaya-cchardi-hidhmāś cānyo-'nya-bheṣajaiḥ ।।

cikitsāsthāna
balino bahu-doṣasya snigdha-svinnasya śodhanam ।
