ūrdhvādho yakṣmiṇaḥ kuryāt sa-snehaṃ yan na karśanam ।।

a-snehaṃ yan na karṣaṇam
payasā phala-yuktena madhureṇa rasena vā ।
sarpiṣ-matyā yavāgvā vā vamana-dravya-siddhayā ।।

vamed virecanaṃ dadyāt trivṛc-chyāmā-nṛpadrumān ।
śarkarā-madhu-sarpirbhiḥ payasā tarpaṇena vā ।।

drākṣā-vidārī-kāśmarya-māṃsānāṃ vā rasair yutān ।
śuddha-koṣṭhasya yuñjīta vidhiṃ bṛṃhaṇa-dīpanam ।।

-māṃsānāṃ vā rasair yutam
hṛdyāni cānna-pānāni vāta-ghnāni laghūni ca ।
śāli-ṣaṣṭika-godhūma-yava-mudgaṃ samoṣitam ।।
laghum a-cyuta-vīryaṃ ca su-jaraṃ bala-kṛc ca yat ।।
laghuṃ cā-cyuta-vīryaṃ ca laghum adbhuta-vīryaṃ ca
ājaṃ kṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ māṃsaṃ kravyān-māṃsaṃ ca śoṣa-jit ।
kākolūka-vṛka-dvīpi-gavāśva-nakuloragam ।।

gṛdhra-bhāsa-kharoṣṭraṃ ca hitaṃ chadmopasaṃhitam ।
jñātaṃ jugupsitaṃ tad dhi cchardiṣe na balaujase ।।

ṛdhra-cāṣa-kharoṣṭraṃ ca
mṛgādyāḥ pitta-kaphayoḥ pavane prasahādayaḥ ।
vesavārī-kṛtāḥ pathyā rasādiṣu ca kalpitāḥ ।।

bhṛṣṭāḥ sarṣapa-tailena sarpiṣā vā yathā-yatham ।
rasikā mṛdavaḥ snigdhāḥ paṭu-dravyābhisaṃskṛtāḥ ।।

hitā maulaka-kaulatthās tad-vad yūṣāś ca sādhitāḥ ।
sa-pippalīkaṃ sa-yavaṃ sa-kulatthaṃ sa-nāgaram ।।

sa-dāḍimaṃ sāmalakaṃ snigdham ājaṃ rasaṃ pibet ।
tena ṣaḍ vinivartante vikārāḥ pīnasādayaḥ ।।

nigdham āja-rasaṃ pibet
pibec ca su-tarāṃ madyaṃ jīrṇaṃ sroto-viśodhanam ।
pittādiṣu viśeṣeṇa madhv-ariṣṭāccha-vāruṇīḥ ।।

adhv-ariṣṭaṃ ca vāruṇīm
siddhaṃ vā pañca-mūlena tāmalakyātha-vā jalam ।
parṇinībhiś catasṛbhir dhānya-nāgarakeṇa vā ।।

kalpayec cānukūlo asya tenānnaṃ śuci yatna-vān ।
daśa-mūlena payasā siddhaṃ māṃsa-rasena vā ।।

balā-garbhaṃ ghṛtaṃ yojyaṃ kravyān-māṃsa-rasena vā ।
sa-kṣaudraṃ payasā siddhaṃ sarpir daśa-guṇena vā ।।

jīvantīṃ madhukaṃ drākṣāṃ phalāni kuṭajasya ca ।
puṣkarāhvaṃ śaṭhīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ vyāghrīṃ gokṣurakaṃ balām ।।

yāghrīṃ gokṣurakaṃ balāḥ
nīlotpalaṃ tāmalakīṃ trāyamāṇāṃ durālabhām ।
kalkī-kṛtya ghṛtaṃ pakvaṃ roga-rāja-haraṃ param ।।

ghṛtaṃ kharjūra-mṛdvīkā-madhukaiḥ sa-parūṣakaiḥ ।
sa-pippalīkaṃ vaisvarya-kāsa-śvāsa-jvarāpaham ।।

daśa-mūla-śṛtāt kṣīrāt sarpir yad udiyān navam ।
sa-pippalīkaṃ sa-kṣaudraṃ tat paraṃ svara-bodhanam ।।

śiraḥ-pārśvāṃsa-śūla-ghnaṃ kāsa-śvāsa-jvarāpaham ।
pañcabhiḥ pañca-mūlair vā śṛtād yad udiyād ghṛtam ।।

pañcānāṃ pañca-mūlānāṃ rase kṣīra-catur-guṇe ।
siddhaṃ sarpir jayaty etad yakṣmaṇaḥ saptakaṃ balam ।।

akṣmiṇaḥ saptakaṃ balam
pañca-kola-yava-kṣāra-ṣaṭ-palena paced ghṛtam ।
prasthonmitaṃ tulya-payaḥ srotasāṃ tad viśodhanam ।।

gulma-jvarodara-plīha-grahaṇī-pāṇḍu-pīnasān ।
śvāsa-kāsāgni-sadana-śvayathūrdhvānilāñ jayet ।।

rāsnā-balā-gokṣuraka-sthirā-varṣābhu-vāriṇi ।
jīvantī-pippalī-garbhaṃ sa-kṣīraṃ śoṣa-jid ghṛtam ।।

aśvagandhā-śṛtāt kṣīrād ghṛtaṃ ca sa-sitā-payaḥ ।
sādhāraṇāmiṣa-tulāṃ toya-droṇa-dvaye pacet ।।

tenāṣṭa-bhāga-śeṣeṇa jīvanīyaiḥ palonmitaiḥ ।
sādhayet sarpiṣaḥ prasthaṃ vāta-pittāmayāpaham ।।

māṃsa-sarpir idam pītaṃ yuktaṃ māṃsa-rasena vā ।
kāsa-śvāsa-svara-bhraṃśa-śoṣa-hṛt-pārśva-śūla-jit ।।

uktaṃ māṃsa-raseṣu vā
elājamodā-tri-phalā-saurāṣṭrī-vyoṣa-citrakān ।
sārān ariṣṭa-gāyatrī-śāla-bījaka-saṃbhavān ।।

bhallātakaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ ca pṛthag aṣṭa-palonmitam ।
salile ṣo-ḍaśa-guṇe ṣo-ḍaśāṃśa-sthitaṃ pacet ।।

punas tena ghṛta-prasthaṃ siddhe cāsmin palāni ṣaṭ ।
tavakṣīryāḥ kṣipet triṃśat sitāyā dvi-guṇaṃ madhu ।।

ghṛtāt tri-jātāt tri-palaṃ tato līḍhaṃ khajāhatam ।
payo-'nu-pānaṃ tat prāhṇe rasāyanam a-yantraṇam ।।

medhyaṃ cakṣuṣyam āyuṣyaṃ dīpanaṃ hanti cā-cirāt ।
meha-gulma-kṣaya-vyādhi-pāṇḍu-roga-bhagandarān ।।

ye ca sarpir-guḍāḥ proktāḥ kṣate yojyāḥ kṣaye api te ।
tvag-elā-pippalī-kṣīrī-śarkarā dvi-guṇāḥ kramāt ।।

cūrṇitā bhakṣitāḥ kṣaudra-sarpiṣā vāvalehitāḥ ।
svaryāḥ kāsa-kṣaya-śvāsa-pārśva-ruk-kapha-nāśanāḥ ।।

-sarpiṣā cāvalehitāḥ
viśeṣāt svara-sāde asya nasya-dhūmādi yojayet ।
tatrāpi vāta-je koṣṇaṃ pibed auttarabhaktikam ।।

ibed uttara-bhaktikam
kāsamardaka-vārtākī-mārkava-sva-rasair ghṛtam ।
sādhitaṃ kāsa-jit svaryaṃ siddham ārtagalena vā ।।

badarī-pattra-kalkaṃ vā ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaṃ sa-saindhavam ।
tailaṃ vā madhuka-drākṣā-pippalī-kṛminut-phalaiḥ ।।

-pippalī-kṛmihṛt-phalaiḥ
haṃsapadyāś ca mūlena pakvaṃ nasto niṣecayet ।
sukhodakānu-pānaṃ ca sa-sarpiṣkaṃ guḍaudanam ।।

aśnīyāt pāyasaṃ caivaṃ snigdhaṃ svedaṃ niyojayet ।
pittodbhave pibet sarpiḥ śṛta-śīta-payo-'nupaḥ ।।

kṣīri-vṛkṣāṅkura-kvātha-kalka-siddhaṃ sa-mākṣikam ।
aśnīyāc ca sa-sarpiṣkaṃ yaṣṭīmadhuka-pāyasam ।।

balā-vidārigandhābhyāṃ vidāryā madhukena ca ।
siddhaṃ sa-lavaṇaṃ sarpir nasyaṃ svaryam an-uttamam ।।

prapauṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ pippalī bṛhatī balā ।
sādhitaṃ kṣīra-sarpiś ca tat svaryaṃ nāvanaṃ param ।।

lihyān madhurakāṇāṃ ca cūrṇaṃ madhu-ghṛtāplutam ।
pibet kaṭūni mūtreṇa kapha-je rūkṣa-bhojanaḥ ।।

kaṭphalāmalaka-vyoṣaṃ lihyāt taila-madhu-plutam ।
vyoṣa-kṣārāgni-cavikā-bhārgī-pathyā-madhūni vā ।।

yavair yavāgūṃ yamake kaṇā-dhātrī-kṛtāṃ pibet ।
bhuktvādyāt pippalīṃ śuṇṭhīṃ tīkṣṇaṃ vā vamanaṃ bhajet ।।

śarkarā-kṣaudra-miśrāṇi śṛtāni madhuraiḥ saha ।
pibet payāṃsi yasyoccair vadato abhihataḥ svaraḥ ।।

vicitram annam a-rucau hitair upahitaṃ hitam ।
bahir-antar-mṛjā citta-nirvāṇaṃ hṛdyam auṣadham ।।

dvau kālau danta-pavanaṃ bhakṣayen mukha-dhāvanaiḥ ।
kaṣāyaiḥ kṣālayed āsyaṃ dhūmaṃ prāyogikaṃ pibet ।।

tālīśa-cūrṇa-vaṭakāḥ sa-karpūra-sitopalāḥ ।
śaśāṅka-kiraṇākhyāś ca bhakṣyā ruci-karāḥ param ।।

hakṣyā ruci-karā bhṛśam
vātād a-rocake tatra pibec cūrṇaṃ prasannayā ।
hareṇu-kṛṣṇā-kṛmijid-drākṣā-saindhava-nāgarāt ।।

elā-bhārgī-yava-kṣāra-hiṅgu-yuktād ghṛtena vā ।
chardayed vā vacāmbhobhiḥ pittāc ca guḍa-vāribhiḥ ।।

lihyād vā śarkarā-sarpir-lavaṇottama-mākṣikam ।
kaphād vamen nimba-jalair dīpyakāragvadhodakam ।।

pānaṃ sa-madhv-ariṣṭāś ca tīkṣṇāḥ sa-madhu-mādhavāḥ ।
pibec cūrṇaṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ hareṇv-ādy-uṣṇa-vāriṇā ।।

elā-tvaṅ-nāgakusuma-tīkṣṇa-kṛṣṇā-mahauṣadham ।
bhāga-vṛddhaṃ kramāc cūrṇaṃ nihanti sama-śarkaram ।।

prasekā-ruci-hṛt-pārśva-kāsa-śvāsa-galāmayān ।
yavānī-tintiḍīkāmla-vetasauṣadha-dāḍimam ।।

kṛtvā kolaṃ ca karṣāṃśaṃ sitāyāś ca catuḥ-palam ।
dhānya-sauvarcalājājī-varāṅgaṃ cārdha-kārṣikam ।।

pippalīnāṃ śataṃ caikaṃ dve śate maricasya ca ।
cūrṇam etat paraṃ rucyaṃ hṛdyaṃ grāhi hinasti ca ।।

ac-cūrṇaṃ dīpanaṃ rucyaṃ
vibandha-kāsa-hṛt-pārśva-plīhārśo-grahaṇī-gadān ।
tālīśa-pattraṃ maricaṃ nāgaraṃ pippalī śubhā ।।

yathottaraṃ bhāga-vṛddhyā tvag-ele cārdha-bhāgike ।
tad rucyaṃ dīpanaṃ cūrṇaṃ kaṇāṣṭa-guṇa-śarkaram ।।

athottaraṃ bhāga-vṛddhās ad dravyaṃ dīpanaṃ cūrṇaṃ
kāsa-śvāsā-ruci-cchardi-plīha-hṛt-pārśva-śūla-nut ।
pāṇḍu-jvarātisāra-ghnaṃ mūḍha-vātānulomanam ।।

arkāmṛtā-kṣāra-jale śarvarīm uṣitair yavaiḥ ।
praseke kalpitān saktūn bhakṣyāṃś cādyād balī vamet ।।

rkāmṛtā-kṣīra-jale
kaṭu-tiktais tathā śūlyaṃ bhakṣayej jāṅgalaṃ palam ।
śuṣkāṃś ca bhakṣyān su-laghūṃś caṇakādi-rasānupaḥ ।।

śleṣmaṇo ati-prasekena vāyuḥ śleṣmāṇam asyati ।
kapha-prasekaṃ taṃ vidvān snigdhoṣṇair eva nirjayet ।।

nigdhoṣṇenaiva nirjayet
pīnase api kramam imaṃ vamathau ca prayojayet ।
viśeṣāt pīnase abhyaṅgān snehān svedāṃś ca śīlayet ।।

īnase ca kramam imaṃ
snigdhān utkārikā-piṇḍaiḥ śiraḥ-pārśva-galādiṣu ।
lavaṇāmla-kaṭūṣṇāṃś ca rasān snehopasaṃhitān ।।

śiro-'ṃsa-pārśva-śūleṣu yathā-doṣa-vidhiṃ caret ।
audakānūpa-piśitair upanāhāḥ su-saṃskṛtāḥ ।।

tatreṣṭāḥ sa-catuḥ-snehā doṣa-saṃsarga iṣyate ।
pralepo nata-yaṣṭy-āhva-śatāhvā-kuṣṭha-candanaiḥ ।।

balā-rāsnā-tilais tad-vat sa-sarpir-madhukotpalaiḥ ।
punarnavā-kṛṣṇagandhā-balā-vīrā-vidāribhiḥ ।।

nāvanaṃ dhūma-pānāni snehāś cauttarabhaktikāḥ ।
tailāny abhyaṅga-yogīni vasti-karma tathā param ।।

śṛṅgādyair vā yathā-doṣaṃ duṣṭam eṣāṃ hared asṛk ।
pradehaḥ sa-ghṛtaiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ padmakośīra-candanaiḥ ।।

dūrvā-madhuka-mañjiṣṭhā-kesarair vā ghṛtāplutaiḥ ।
vaṭādi-siddha-tailena śata-dhautena sarpiṣā ।।

abhyaṅgaḥ payasā sekaḥ śastaś ca madhukāmbunā ।
prāyeṇopahatāgni-tvāt sa-piccham atisāryate ।।

tasyātīsāra-grahaṇī-vihitaṃ hitam auṣadham ।
purīṣaṃ yatnato rakṣec chuṣyato rāja-yakṣmiṇaḥ ।।

sarva-dhātu-kṣayārtasya balaṃ tasya hi viḍ-balam ।
māṃsam evāśnato yuktyā mārdvīkaṃ pibato anu ca ।।

a-vidhārita-vegasya yakṣmā na labhate antaram ।
surāṃ sa-maṇḍāṃ mārdvīkam ariṣṭān sīdhu-mādhavān ।।

riṣṭaṃ sīdhu-mādhavān
yathārham anu-pānārthaṃ piben māṃsāni bhakṣayan ।
sroto-vibandha-mokṣārthaṃ balaujaḥ-puṣṭaye ca tat ।।

sneha-kṣīrāmbu-koṣṭheṣu sv-abhyaktam avagāhayet ।
uttīrṇaṃ miśrakaiḥ snehair bhūyo abhyaktaṃ sukhaiḥ karaiḥ ।।

ttīrṇaṃ miśraka-snehair
mṛdnīyāt sukham āsīnaṃ sukhaṃ codvartayet param ।
jīvantīṃ śatavīryāṃ ca vikasāṃ sa-punarnavām ।।

aśvagandhām apāmārgaṃ tarkārīṃ madhukaṃ balām ।
vidārīṃ sarṣapān kuṣṭhaṃ taṇḍulān atasī-phalam ।।

māṣāṃs tilāṃś ca kiṇvaṃ ca sarvam eka-tra cūrṇayet ।
yava-cūrṇaṃ tri-guṇitaṃ dadhnā yuktaṃ sa-mākṣikam ।।

etad udvartanaṃ kāryaṃ puṣṭi-varṇa-bala-pradam ।
gaura-sarṣapa-kalkena snānīyauṣadhibhiś ca saḥ ।।

tad utsādanaṃ kāryaṃ nānair auṣadhibhiś ca saḥ
snāyād ṛtu-sukhais toyair jīvanīyopasādhitaiḥ ।
gandha-mālyādikāṃ bhūṣām a-lakṣmī-nāśanīṃ bhajet ।।

andha-mālyādikair bhūṣām
suhṛdāṃ darśanaṃ gīta-vāditrotsava-saṃśrutiḥ ।
vastayaḥ kṣīra-sarpīṃṣi madya-māṃsa-su-śīla-tā ।।

adyaṃ māṃsaṃ su-śīla-tā daiva-vyapāśrayaṃ tat tad atharvoktaṃ ca pūjitam ।।

cikitsāsthāna
āmāśayotkleśa-bhavāḥ prāyaś chardyo hitaṃ tataḥ ।
laṅghanaṃ prāg ṛte vāyor vamanaṃ tatra yojayet ।।

rāyaś chardyo hitaṃ matam
balino bahu-doṣasya vamataḥ pratataṃ bahu ।
tato virekaṃ krama-śo hṛdyaṃ madyaiḥ phalāmbubhiḥ ।।

kṣīrair vā saha sa hy ūrdhvaṃ gataṃ doṣaṃ nayaty adhaḥ ।
śamanaṃ cauṣadhaṃ rūkṣa-dur-balasya tad eva tu ।।

pariśuṣkaṃ priyaṃ sātmyam annaṃ laghu ca śasyate ।
upavāsas tathā yūṣā rasāḥ kāmbalikāḥ khalāḥ ।।

śākāni lehā bhojyāni rāga-ṣāḍava-pānakāḥ ।
bhakṣyāḥ śuṣkā vicitrāś ca phalāni snāna-gharṣaṇam ।।

gandhāḥ su-gandhayo gandha-phala-puṣpānna-pāna-jāḥ ।
bhukta-mātrasya sahasā mukhe śītāmbu-secanam ।।

hanti māruta-jāṃ chardiṃ sarpiḥ pītaṃ sa-saindhavam ।
kiñ-cid-uṣṇaṃ viśeṣeṇa sa-kāsa-hṛdaya-dravām ।।

vyoṣa-tri-lavaṇāḍhyaṃ vā siddhaṃ vā dāḍimāmbunā ।
sa-śuṇṭhī-dadhi-dhānyena śṛtaṃ tulyāmbu vā payaḥ ।।

śṛtaṃ tulyāmbunā payaḥ ītaṃ tulyāmbunā payaḥ
vyakta-saindhava-sarpir vā phalāmlo vaiṣkiro rasaḥ ।
snigdhaṃ ca bhojanaṃ śuṇṭhī-dadhi-dāḍima-sādhitam ।।

koṣṇaṃ sa-lavaṇaṃ cātra hitaṃ sneha-virecanam ।
pitta-jāyāṃ virekārthaṃ drākṣekṣu-sva-rasais trivṛt ।।

sarpir vā tailvakaṃ yojyaṃ vṛddhaṃ ca śleṣma-dhāma-gam ।
ūrdhvam eva haret pittaṃ svādu-tiktair viśuddhi-mān ।।

piben manthaṃ yavāgūṃ vā lājaiḥ sa-madhu-śarkarām ।
mudga-jāṅgala-jair adyād vyañjanaiḥ śāli-ṣaṣṭikam ।।

ājaiḥ sa-madhu-śarkaraiḥ
mṛd-bhṛṣṭa-loṣṭa-prabhavaṃ su-śītaṃ salilaṃ pibet ।
mudgośīra-kaṇā-dhānyaiḥ saha vā saṃsthitaṃ niśām ।।

drākṣā-rasaṃ rasaṃ vekṣor guḍūcy-ambu payo api vā ।
jambv-āmra-pallavośīra-vaṭa-śuṅgāvaroha-jaḥ ।।

rākṣā-rasaṃ rasaṃ cekṣor -vaṭa-śṛṅgāvaroha-jaḥ
kvāthaḥ kṣaudra-yutaḥ pītaḥ śīto vā viniyacchati ।
chardiṃ jvaram atīsāraṃ mūrchāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ ca dur-jayām ।।

dhātrī-rasena vā śītaṃ piben mudga-dalāmbu vā ।
kola-majja-sitā-lājā-makṣikā-viṭ-kaṇāñjanam ।।

ola-majja-sitā-lākṣā- -makṣikā-viṭ-rasāñjanam
lihyāt kṣaudreṇa pathyāṃ vā drākṣāṃ vā badarāṇi vā ।
kapha-jāyāṃ vamen nimba-kṛṣṇā-piṇḍīta-sarṣapaiḥ ।।

yuktena koṣṇa-toyena dur-balaṃ copavāsayet ।
āragvadhādi-niryūhaṃ śītaṃ kṣaudra-yutaṃ pibet ।।

āragvadhāder niryūhaṃ
manthān yavair vā bahu-śaś chardi-ghnauṣadha-bhāvitaiḥ ।
kapha-ghnam annaṃ hṛdyaṃ ca rāgāḥ sārjaka-bhūstṛṇāḥ ।।

līḍhaṃ manaḥśilā-kṛṣṇā-maricaṃ bījapūrakāt ।
sva-rasena kapitthasya sa-kṣaudreṇa vamiṃ jayet ।।

khādet kapitthaṃ sa-vyoṣaṃ madhunā vā durālabhām ।
lihyān marica-cocailā-go-śakṛd-rasa-mākṣikam ।।

anukūlopacāreṇa yāti dviṣṭārtha-jā śamam ।
kṛmi-jā kṛmi-hṛd-roga-gaditaiś ca bhiṣag-jitaiḥ ।।
yathā-svaṃ pariśeṣāś ca tat-kṛtāś ca tathāmayāḥ ।।
chardi-prasaṅgena hi mātariśvā dhātu-kṣayāt kopam upaity avaśyam ।
kuryād ato asmin vamanāti-yoga-proktaṃ vidhiṃ stambhana-bṛṃhaṇīyam ।।

uryād ato asmin vamanāti-yoge roktaṃ vidhiṃ 
stambhana-bṛṃhaṇīyam
sarpir-guḍā māṃsa-rasā ghṛtāni kalyāṇaka-try-ūṣaṇa-jīvanāni ।
payāṃsi pathyopahitāni lehāś chardiṃ prasaktāṃ praśamaṃ nayanti ।।

arpir guḍo māṃsa-rasā ghṛtāni iti chardi-cikitsitam atha hṛd-roga-cikitsitam ।।
hṛd-roge vāta-je tailaṃ mastu-sauvīra-takra-vat ।।tailaṃ ca lavaṇaiḥ siddhaṃ sa-mūtrāmlaṃ tathā-guṇam ।।
pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ sa-viḍaṃ gulmānāhārti-jic ca tat ।
tailaṃ ca lavaṇaiḥ siddhaṃ sa-mūtrāmlaṃ tathā-guṇam ।।

bilvaṃ rāsnāṃ yavān kolaṃ devadāruṃ punarnavām ।
kulatthān pañca-mūlaṃ ca paktvā tasmin pacej jale ।।

tailaṃ tan nāvane pāne vastau ca viniyojayet ।
śuṇṭhī-vayaḥsthā-lavaṇa-kāyasthā-hiṅgu-pauṣkaraiḥ ।।

śuṇṭhī-kayasthā-lavaṇa- -vayaḥsthā-hiṅgu-pauṣkaraiḥ
pathyayā ca śṛtaṃ pārśva-hṛd-rujā-gulma-jid ghṛtam ।
sauvarcalasya dvi-pale pathyā-pañcāśad-anvite ।।

ghṛtasya sādhitaḥ prastho hṛd-roga-śvāsa-gulma-jit ।
dāḍimaṃ kṛṣṇa-lavaṇaṃ śuṇṭhī-hiṅgv-amla-vetasam ।।

ṛd-roga-śvāsa-gulma-hṛt śuṇṭhī hiṅgv amla-vetasaḥ
apatantraka-hṛd-roga-śvāsa-ghnaṃ cūrṇam uttamam ।
puṣkarāhva-śaṭhī-śuṇṭhī-bījapūra-jaṭābhayāḥ ।।

pītāḥ kalkī-kṛtāḥ kṣāra-ghṛtāmla-lavaṇair yutāḥ ।
vikartikā-śūla-harāḥ kvāthaḥ koṣṇaś ca tad-guṇaḥ ।।

yavānī-lavaṇa-kṣāra-vacājājy-auṣadhaiḥ kṛtaḥ ।
sa-pūtidāru-bījāhva-palāśa-śaṭhi-pauṣkaraiḥ ।।

a pūtidāru-bījāhva- -vijayā-śaṭhi-pauṣkaraiḥ
yava-kṣāro yavānī ca pibed uṣṇena vāriṇā ।
etena vāta-jaṃ śūlaṃ gulmaṃ caiva cirotthitam ।।
bhidyate sapta-rātreṇa pavanena yathā ghanaḥ ।।
pañca-kola-śaṭhī-pathyā-guḍa-bījāhva-pauṣkaram ।
vāruṇī-kalkitaṃ bhṛṣṭaṃ yamake lavaṇānvitam ।।

hṛt-pārśva-yoni-śūleṣu khāded gulmodareṣu ca ।
snigdhāś ceha hitāḥ svedāḥ saṃskṛtāni ghṛtāni ca ।।

aṃskṛtāni ghṛtāni tu
laghunā pañca-mūlena śuṇṭhyā vā sādhitaṃ jalam ।
vāruṇī-dadhi-maṇḍaṃ vā dhānyāmlaṃ vā pibet tṛṣi ।।

āruṇīṃ dadhi-maṇḍaṃ vā
sāyāma-stambha-śūlāme hṛdi māruta-dūṣite ।
kriyaiṣā sa-dravāyāma-pramohe tu hitā rasāḥ ।।

snehāḍhyās tittiri-krauñca-śikhi-vartaka-dakṣa-jāḥ ।
balā-tailaṃ sa-hṛd-rogaḥ pibed vā su-kumārakam ।।

nehādyās tittiri-krauñca-
yaṣṭy-āhva-śata-pākaṃ vā mahā-snehaṃ tathottamam ।
rāsnā-jīvaka-jīvantī-balā-vyāghrī-punarnavaiḥ ।।

bhārgī-sthirā-vacā-vyoṣair mahā-snehaṃ vipācayet ।
dadhi-pādaṃ tathāmlaiś ca lābhataḥ sa niṣevitaḥ ।।

tarpaṇo bṛṃhaṇo balyo vāta-hṛd-roga-nāśanaḥ ।
dīpte agnau sa-dravāyāme hṛd-roge vātike hitam ।।

kṣīraṃ dadhi guḍaḥ sarpir audakānūpam āmiṣam ।
etāny eva ca varjyāni hṛd-rogeṣu caturṣv api ।।

śeṣeṣu stambha-jāḍyāma-saṃyukte api ca vātike ।
kaphānubandhe tasmiṃs tu rūkṣoṣṇām ācaret kriyām ।।

paitte drākṣekṣu-niryāsa-sitā-kṣaudra-parūṣakaiḥ ।
yukto vireko hṛdyaḥ syāt kramaḥ śuddhe ca pitta-hā ।।

ukto vireco hṛdyaḥ syāt
kṣata-pitta-jvaroktaṃ ca bāhyāntaḥ parimārjanam ।
kaṭvī-madhuka-kalkaṃ ca pibet sa-sitam ambhasā ।।

śreyasī-śarkarā-drākṣā-jīvakarṣabhakotpalaiḥ ।
balā-kharjūra-kākolī-medā-yugmaiś ca sādhitam ।।

sa-kṣīraṃ māhiṣaṃ sarpiḥ pitta-hṛd-roga-nāśanam ।
prapauṇḍarīka-madhuka-bisa-granthi-kaserukāḥ ।।

sa-śuṇṭhī-śaivalās tābhiḥ sa-kṣīraṃ vipaced ghṛtam ।
śītaṃ sa-madhu tac ceṣṭaṃ svādu-varga-kṛtaṃ ca yat ।।

vastiṃ ca dadyāt sa-kṣaudraṃ tailaṃ madhuka-sādhitam ।
kaphodbhave vamet svinnaḥ picumanda-vacāmbhasā ।।

astiṃ ca dadyāt sa-kṣaudra- -tailaṃ madhuka-sādhitam 
picumanda-vacāmbunā
kulattha-dhanvottha-rasa-tīkṣṇa-madya-yavāśanaḥ ।
pibec cūrṇaṃ vacā-hiṅgu-lavaṇa-dvaya-nāgarāt ।।

sailā-yavānaka-kaṇā-yava-kṣārāt sukhāmbunā ।
phala-dhānyāmla-kaulattha-yūṣa-mūtrāsavais tathā ।।

ailā-yavānika-kaṇā-
puṣkarāhvābhayā-śuṇṭhī-śaṭhī-rāsnā-vacā-kaṇāt ।
kvāthaṃ tathābhayā-śuṇṭhī-mādrī-pītadru-kaṭphalāt ।।

c -śaṭhī-rāsnā-vacā-kaṇā- c -kvāthaṃ tathābhayā-śuṇṭhī-
kvāthe rohītakāśvattha-khadirodumbarārjune ।
sa-palāśa-vaṭe vyoṣa-trivṛc-cūrṇānvite kṛtaḥ ।।

sukhodakānu-pānaś ca lehaḥ kapha-vikāra-hā ।
śleṣma-gulmoditājyāni kṣārāṃś ca vividhān pibet ।।

ukhodakānu-pānasya
prayojayec chilāhvaṃ vā brāhmaṃ vātra rasāyanam ।
tathāmalaka-lehaṃ vā prāśaṃ vāgastya-nirmitam ।।

rāhmaṃ cātra rasāyanam rāśyaṃ vāgastya-nirmitam 
prāśyaṃ cāgastya-nirmitam
syāc chūlaṃ yasya bhukte ati jīryaty alpaṃ jarāṃ gate ।
śāmyet sa kuṣṭha-kṛmijil-lavaṇa-dvaya-tilvakaiḥ ।।

yāc chūlaṃ yasya bhukte anne
sa-devadārv-ativiṣaiś cūrṇam uṣṇāmbunā pibet ।
yasya jīrṇe adhikaṃ snehaiḥ sa virecyaḥ phalaiḥ punaḥ ।।

jīryaty anne tathā mūlais tīkṣṇaiḥ śūle sadādhike ।
prāyo anilo ruddha-gatiḥ kupyaty āmāśaye gataḥ ।।

upyaty āmāśaye tataḥ upyaty āmāśaye yataḥ
tasyānulomanaṃ kāryaṃ śuddhi-laṅghana-pācanaiḥ ।
kṛmi-ghnam auṣadhaṃ sarvaṃ kṛmi-je hṛdayāmaye ।।

ṛmi-je ca hṛd-āmaye
tṛṣṇāsu vāta-pitta-ghno vidhiḥ prāyeṇa śasyate ।
sarvāsu śīto bāhyāntas tathā śamana-śodhanaḥ ।।

idhiḥ prāyeṇa yujyate athā śamana-śodhanam
divyāmbu śītaṃ sa-kṣaudraṃ tad-vad bhaumaṃ ca tad-guṇam ।
nirvāpitaṃ tapta-loṣṭa-kapāla-sikatādibhiḥ ।।

sa-śarkaraṃ vā kvathitaṃ pañca-mūlena vā jalam ।
darbha-pūrveṇa manthaś ca praśasto lāja-saktubhiḥ ।।

vāṭyaś cāma-yavaiḥ śītaḥ śarkarā-mākṣikānvitaḥ ।
yavāgūḥ śālibhis tad-vat kodravaiś ca ciran-tanaiḥ ।।

śītena śīta-vīryaiś ca dravyaiḥ siddhena bhojanam ।
himāmbu-pariṣiktasya payasā sa-sitā-madhu ।।

rasaiś cān-amla-lavaṇair jāṅgalair ghṛta-bharjitaiḥ ।
mudgādīnāṃ tathā yūṣair jīvanīya-rasānvitaiḥ ।।

asaiś cān-alpa-lavaṇair
nasyaṃ kṣīra-ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ śītair ikṣos tathā rasaḥ ।
nirvāpaṇāś ca gaṇḍūṣāḥ sūtra-sthānoditā hitāḥ ।।

śītair ikṣos tathā rasaiḥ śītair ikṣos tathā rase
dāha-jvaroktā lepādyā nirīha-tvaṃ mano-ratiḥ ।
mahā-sarid-dhradādīnāṃ darśana-smaraṇāni ca ।।

arśana-smaraṇādi ca
tṛṣṇāyāṃ pavanotthāyāṃ sa-guḍaṃ dadhi śasyate ।
rasāś ca bṛṃhaṇāḥ śītā vidāry-ādi-gaṇāmbu ca ।।

idāry-ādi-gaṇāmbu vā
pitta-jāyāṃ sitā-yuktaḥ pakvodumbara-jo rasaḥ ।
tat-kvātho vā himas tad-vac chārivādi-gaṇāmbu vā ।।

tad-vidhaiś ca gaṇaiḥ śīta-kaṣāyān sa-sitā-madhūn ।
madhurair auṣadhais tad-vat kṣīri-vṛkṣaiś ca kalpitān ।।

bījapūraka-mṛdvīkā-vaṭa-vetasa-pallavān ।
mūlāni kuśa-kāśānāṃ yaṣṭy-āhvaṃ ca jale śṛtam ।।

jvaroditaṃ vā drākṣādi pañca-sārāmbu vā pibet ।
kaphodbhavāyāṃ vamanaṃ nimba-prasava-vāriṇā ।।

bilvāḍhakī-pañca-kola-darbha-pañcaka-sādhitam ।
jalaṃ pibed rajanyā vā siddhaṃ sa-kṣaudra-śarkaram ।।

-darbha-kacchaka-sādhitam alaṃ pibed rajanyāṃ vā
mudga-yūṣaṃ ca sa-vyoṣa-paṭolī-nimba-pallavam ।
yavānnaṃ tīkṣṇa-kavaḍa-nasya-lehāṃś ca śīlayet ।।

sarvair āmāc ca tad dhantrī kriyeṣṭā vamanaṃ tathā ।
try-ūṣaṇāruṣkara-vacā-phalāmloṣṇāmbu-mastubhiḥ ।।

annātyayān maṇḍam uṣṇaṃ himaṃ manthaṃ ca kāla-vit ।
tṛṣi śramān māṃsa-rasaṃ manthaṃ vā sa-sitaṃ pibet ।।

adyaṃ vā sa-sitaṃ pibet
ātapāt sa-sitaṃ manthaṃ yava-kola-ja-saktubhiḥ ।
sarvāṇy aṅgāni limpec ca tila-piṇyāka-kāñjikaiḥ ।।

śīta-snānāc ca madyāmbu pibet tṛṇ-mān guḍāmbu vā ।
madyād ardha-jalaṃ madyaṃ snāto amla-lavaṇair yutam ।।

śīta-snānāt tu madyāmbu ibet tṛḍ-vān guḍāmbu vā 
snāto amla-lavaṇāyutam
sneha-tīkṣṇa-tarāgnis tu sva-bhāva-śiśiraṃ jalam ।
snehād uṣṇāma-jīrṇāt tu jīrṇān maṇḍaṃ pipāsitaḥ ।।

nehāt tīkṣṇa-tarāgnis tu
pibet snigdhānna-tṛṣito hima-spardhi guḍodakam ।
gurv-ādy-annena tṛṣitaḥ pītvoṣṇāmbu tad ullikhet ।।

kṣaya-jāyāṃ kṣaya-hitaṃ sarvaṃ bṛṃhaṇam auṣadham ।
kṛśa-dur-bala-rūkṣāṇāṃ kṣīraṃ chāgo raso atha-vā ।।

kṣīraṃ ca sordhva-vātāyāṃ kṣaya-kāsa-haraiḥ śṛtam ।
rogopasargāj jātāyāṃ dhānyāmbu sa-sitā-madhu ।।

ogopasarga-jātāyāṃ
pāne praśastaṃ sarvā ca kriyā rogādy-apekṣayā ।
tṛṣyan pūrvāmaya-kṣīṇo na labheta jalaṃ yadi ।।

ṛṣṇan pūrvāmaya-kṣīṇo c tṛṣṇak pūrvāmaya-kṣīṇo
maraṇaṃ dīrgha-rogaṃ vā prāpnuyāt tvaritaṃ tataḥ ।
sātmyānna-pāna-bhaiṣajyais tṛṣṇāṃ tasya jayet purā ।।

ṛṣṇāṃ tasya jayet puras tasyāṃ jitāyām anyo api vyādhiḥ śakyaś cikitsitum ।।

cikitsāsthāna
yaṃ doṣam adhikaṃ paśyet tasyādau pratikārayet ।
kapha-sthānānupūrvyā ca tulya-doṣe madātyaye ।।

apha-sthānānupūrvyā tu
pitta-māruta-pary-antaḥ prāyeṇa hi madātyayaḥ ।
hīna-mithyāti-pītena yo vyādhir upajāyate ।।

sama-pītena tenaiva sa madyenopaśāmyati ।
madyasya viṣa-sādṛśyād viṣaṃ tūtkarṣa-vṛttibhiḥ ।।

tīkṣṇādibhir guṇair yogād viṣāntaram apekṣate ।
tīkṣṇoṣṇenāti-mātreṇa pītenāmla-vidāhinā ।।

madyenānna-rasa-kledo vidagdhaḥ kṣāra-tāṃ gataḥ ।
yān kuryān mada-tṛṇ-moha-jvarāntar-dāha-vibhramān ।।

madyotkliṣṭena doṣeṇa ruddhaḥ srotaḥsu mārutaḥ ।
su-tīvrā vedanā yāś ca śirasy asthiṣu saṃdhiṣu ।।

jīrṇāma-madya-doṣasya prakāṅkṣā-lāghave sati ।
yaugikaṃ vidhi-vad yuktaṃ madyam eva nihanti tān ।।

kṣāro hi yāti mādhuryaṃ śīghram amlopasaṃhitaḥ ।
madyam amleṣu ca śreṣṭhaṃ doṣa-viṣyandanād alam ।।

oṣa-visrāvaṇād alam
tīkṣṇoṣṇādyaiḥ purā proktair dīpanādyais tathā guṇaiḥ ।
sātmya-tvāc ca tad evāsya dhātu-sāmya-karaṃ param ।।

saptāham aṣṭa-rātraṃ vā kuryāt pānātyayauṣadham ।
jīryaty etāvatā pānaṃ kālena vi-pathāśritam ।।

paraṃ tato anubadhnāti yo rogas tasya bheṣajam ।
yathā-yathaṃ prayuñjīta kṛta-pānātyayauṣadhaḥ ।।

ṛta-pānātyayauṣadham
tatra vātolbaṇe madyaṃ dadyāt piṣṭa-kṛtaṃ yutam ।
bījapūraka-vṛkṣāmla-kola-dāḍima-dīpyakaiḥ ।।

yavānī-hapuṣājājī-vyoṣa-tri-lavaṇārdrakaiḥ ।
śūlya-māṃsair harītakaiḥ sneha-vadbhiś ca saktubhiḥ ।।

-vyoṣa-tri-lavaṇārjakaiḥ śūlya-māṃsair haritakaiḥ
uṣṇa-snigdhāmla-lavaṇā medya-māṃsa-rasā hitāḥ ।
āmrāmrātaka-peśībhiḥ saṃskṛtā rāga-ṣāḍavāḥ ।।

ṣṇāḥ snigdhāmla-lavaṇā adya-māṃsa-rasā hitāḥ 
saṃskṛtā rāga-khāṇḍavāḥ
godhūma-māṣa-vikṛtir mṛduś citrā mukha-priyā ।
ārdrikārdraka-kulmāṣa-śukta-māṃsādi-garbhiṇī ।।

surabhir lavaṇā śītā nir-gadā vāccha-vāruṇī ।
sva-raso dāḍimāt kvāthaḥ pañca-mūlāt kanīyasaḥ ।।

igadā vāccha-vāruṇī
śuṇṭhī-dhānyāt tathā mastu śuktāmbho-'cchāmla-kāñjikam ।
abhyaṅgodvartana-snānam uṣṇaṃ prāvaraṇaṃ ghanam ।।

ghanaś cāguru-jo dhūpaḥ paṅkaś cāguru-kuṅkumaḥ ।
kucoru-śroṇi-śālinyo yauvanoṣṇāṅga-yaṣṭayaḥ ।।

harṣeṇāliṅgane yuktāḥ priyāḥ saṃvāhaneṣu ca ।
pittolbaṇe bahu-jalaṃ śārkaraṃ madhu vā yutam ।।

rasair dāḍima-kharjūra-bhavya-drākṣā-parūṣa-jaiḥ ।
su-śītaṃ sa-sitā-saktu yojyaṃ tādṛk ca pānakam ।।

-bhavya-drākṣā-parūṣakaiḥ -paṭolī-dāḍimair api
svādu-varga-kaṣāyair vā yuktaṃ madyaṃ sa-mākṣikam ।
śāli-ṣaṣṭikam aśnīyāc chaśājaiṇa-kapiñjalaiḥ ।।

satīna-mudgāmalaka-paṭolī-dāḍimai rasaiḥ ।
kapha-pittaṃ samutkliṣṭam ullikhet tṛḍ-vidāha-vān ।।

pītvāmbu śītaṃ madyaṃ vā bhūrīkṣu-rasa-saṃyutam ।
drākṣā-rasaṃ vā saṃsargī tarpaṇādiḥ paraṃ hitaḥ ।।

tathāgnir dīpyate tasya doṣa-śeṣānna-pācanaḥ ।
kāse sa-rakta-niṣṭhīve pārśva-stana-rujāsu ca ।।

tṛṣṇāyāṃ sa-vidāhāyāṃ sotkleśe hṛdayorasi ।
guḍūcī-bhadra-mustānāṃ paṭolasyātha-vā rasam ।।

sa-śṛṅgaveraṃ yuñjīta tittiri-pratibhojanam ।
tṛṣyate cāti bala-vad vāta-pitte samuddhate ।।

a-nāgaraṃ yojayeta
dadyād drākṣā-rasaṃ pānaṃ śītaṃ doṣānulomanam ।
jīrṇe adyān madhurāmlena cchāga-māṃsa-rasena ca ।।

tṛṣy alpa-śaḥ piben madyaṃ madaṃ rakṣan bahūdakam ।
musta-dāḍima-lājāmbu jalaṃ vā parṇinī-śṛtam ।।

pāṭaly-utpala-kandair vā sva-bhāvād eva vā himam ।
madyāti-pānād ab-dhātau kṣīṇe tejasi coddhate ।।

aṭoly-utpala-kandair vā
yaḥ śuṣka-gala-tālv-oṣṭho jihvāṃ niṣkṛṣya ceṣṭate ।
pāyayet kāmato ambhas taṃ niśītha-pavanāhatam ।।

kola-dāḍima-vṛkṣāmla-cukrīkā-cukrikā-rasaḥ ।
pañcāmlako mukhālepaḥ sadyas tṛṣṇāṃ niyacchati ।।

tvacaṃ prāptaś ca pānoṣmā pitta-raktābhimūrchitaḥ ।
dāhaṃ prakurute ghoraṃ tatrāti-śiśiro vidhiḥ ।।

vacaṃ prāptas tu pānoṣmā vacaṃ prāptaḥ sa pānoṣmā
a-śāmyati rasais tṛpte rohiṇīṃ vyadhayet sirām ।
ullekhanopavāsābhyāṃ jayec chleṣmolbaṇaṃ pibet ।।

śītaṃ śuṇṭhī-sthirodīcya-duḥsparśānya-tamodakam ।
nir-āmaṃ kṣudhitaṃ kāle pāyayed bahu-mākṣikam ।।

śārkaraṃ madhu vā jīrṇam ariṣṭaṃ sīdhum eva vā ।
rūkṣa-tarpaṇa-saṃyuktaṃ yavānī-nāgarānvitam ।।

yūṣeṇa yava-godhūmaṃ tanunālpena bhojayet ।
uṣṇāmla-kaṭu-tiktena kaulatthenālpa-sarpiṣā ।।

ṣṇāmbu-kaṭu-tiktena
śuṣka-mūlaka-jaiś chāgai rasair vā dhanva-cāriṇām ।
sāmla-vetasa-vṛkṣāmla-paṭolī-vyoṣa-dāḍimaiḥ ।।

-pāṭalī-vyoṣa-dāḍimaiḥ
prabhūta-śuṇṭhī-marica-haritārdraka-peśikam ।
bījapūra-rasādy-amla-bhṛṣṭa-nī-rasa-vartitam ।।

karīra-karamardādi rociṣṇu bahu-śālanam ।
pravyaktāṣṭāṅga-lavaṇaṃ vikalpita-nimardakam ।।

ikalpita-vimardakam
yathāgni bhakṣayan māṃsaṃ mādhavaṃ nigadaṃ pibet ।
sitā-sauvarcalājājī-tintiḍīkāmla-vetasam ।।

ādhavaṃ nir-gadaṃ pibet
tvag-elā-maricārdhāṃśam aṣṭāṅga-lavaṇaṃ hitam ।
sroto-viśuddhy-agni-karaṃ kapha-prāye madātyaye ।।

rūkṣoṣṇodvartanodgharṣa-snāna-bhojana-laṅghanaiḥ ।
sa-kāmābhiḥ saha strībhir yuktyā jāgaraṇena ca ।।

madātyayaḥ kapha-prāyaḥ śīghraṃ samupaśāmyati ।
yad idaṃ karma nirdiṣṭaṃ pṛthag doṣa-balaṃ prati ।।

saṃnipāte daśa-vidhe tac cheṣe api vikalpayet ।
tvaṅ-nāgapuṣpa-magadhā-maricājāji-dhānyakaiḥ ।।

parūṣaka-madhūkailā-surāhvaiś ca sitānvitaiḥ ।
sa-kapittha-rasaṃ hṛdyaṃ pānakaṃ śaśi-bodhitam ।।

madātyayeṣu sarveṣu peyaṃ rucy-agni-dīpanam ।
nā-vikṣobhya mano madyaṃ śarīram a-vihanya vā ।।

ā-kṣobhya hi mano madyaṃ śarīram a-vihatya vā
kuryān madātyayaṃ tasmād iṣyate harṣaṇī kriyā ।
saṃśuddhi-śamanādyeṣu mada-doṣaḥ kṛteṣv api ।।

na cec chāmyet kaphe kṣīṇe jāte daurbalya-lāghave ।
tasya madya-vidagdhasya vāta-pittādhikasya ca ।।

grīṣmopataptasya taror yathā varṣaṃ tathā payaḥ ।
madya-kṣīṇasya hi kṣīṇaṃ kṣīram āśv eva puṣyati ।।

adya-kṣīṇasya hi kṣīraṃ ītam āśv eva puṣyati
ojas tulyaṃ guṇaiḥ sarvair viparītaṃ ca madyataḥ ।
payasā vihate roge bale jāte nivartayet ।।

ayasā vijite roge
kṣīra-prayogaṃ madyaṃ ca krameṇālpālpam ācaret ।
na vikṣaya-dhvaṃsakotthaiḥ spṛśetopadravair yathā ।।

a viṭ-kṣaya-dhvaṃsakotthaiḥ pṛśyetopadravair yathā
tayos tu syād ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ vastayo bṛṃhaṇāḥ śivāḥ ।
abhyaṅgodvartana-snānāny anna-pānaṃ ca vāta-jit ।।

yukta-madyasya madyottho na vyādhir upajāyate ।
ato asya vakṣyate yogo yaḥ sukhāyaiva kevalam ।।

āśvinaṃ yā mahat tejo balaṃ sārasvataṃ ca yā ।
dadhāty aindraṃ ca yā vīryaṃ prabhāvaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca yā ।।

astraṃ makara-ketor yā puruṣārtho balasya yā ।
sautrāmaṇyāṃ dvi-ja-mukhe yā hutāśe ca hvayate ।।

uruṣārtho balasya ca
yā sarvauṣadhi-saṃpūrṇān mathyamānāt surāsuraiḥ ।
mahoda-dheḥ samudbhūtā śrī-śaśāṅkāmṛtaiḥ saha ।।

madhu-mādhava-maireya-sīdhu-gauḍāsavādibhiḥ ।
mada-śaktim an-ujjhantī yā rūpair bahubhiḥ sthitā ।।

ada-śaktim a-tyajantī
yām āsvādya vilāsinyo yathārthaṃ nāma bibhrati ।
kulāṅganāpi yāṃ pītvā nayaty uddhata-mānasā ।।

ām āsādya vilāsinyo
an-aṅgāliṅgitair aṅgaiḥ kvāpi ceto muner api ।
taraṅga-bhaṅga-bhrū-kuṭī-tarjanair māninī-manaḥ ।।

ekaṃ prasādya kurute yā dvayor api nirvṛtim ।
yathā-kāmaṃ bhaṭāvāpti-parihṛṣṭāpsaro-gaṇe ।।

athā-kāma-bhaṭāvāpti-
tṛṇa-vat puruṣā yuddhe yām āsvādya tyajanty asūn ।
yāṃ śīlayitvāpi ciraṃ bahu-dhā bahu-vigrahām ।।

ām āsādya tyajanty asūn
nityaṃ harṣāti-vegena tat-pūrvam iva sevate ।
śokodvegā-rati-bhayair yāṃ dṛṣṭvā nābhibhūyate ।।

goṣṭhī-mahotsavodyānaṃ na yasyāḥ śobhate vinā ।
smṛtvā smṛtvā ca bahu-śo viyuktaḥ śocate yayā ।।

mṛtvā tu yāṃ ca bahu-śo
a-prasannāpi yā prītyai prasannā svarga eva yā ।
apīndraṃ manyate duḥ-sthaṃ hṛdaya-sthitayā yayā ।।

a-nirdeśya-sukhāsvādā svayaṃ-vedyaiva yā param ।
iti citrāsv avasthāsu priyām anukaroti yā ।।

priyāti-priya-tāṃ yāti yat priyasya viśeṣataḥ ।
yā prītir yā ratir vā vāg yā puṣṭir iti ca stutā ।।

deva-dānava-gandharva-yakṣa-rākṣasa-mānuṣaiḥ ।
pāna-pravṛttau satyāṃ tu tāṃ surāṃ vidhinā pibet ।।

-yakṣa-rākṣasa-mānavaiḥ -yakṣa-rākṣasa-mānavaiḥ
saṃbhavanti na te rogā medo-'nila-kaphodbhavāḥ ।
vidhi-yuktād ṛte madyād ye na sidhyanti dāruṇāḥ ।।

aṃbhavanti ca ye rogā idhi-yuktād ṛte madyāt e na 
sidhyanti dāruṇāḥ
asti dehasya sāvasthā yasyāṃ pānaṃ nivāryate ।
anya-tra madyān nigadād vividhauṣadha-saṃskṛtāt ।।

ividhauṣadha-saṃbhṛtāt
ānūpaṃ jāṅgalaṃ ṃāṃsaṃ vidhināpy upakalpitam ।
madyaṃ sahāyam a-prāpya samyak pariṇamet katham ।।

su-tīvra-māruta-vyādhi-ghātino laśunasya ca ।
madya-māṃsa-viyuktasya prayoge syāt kiyān guṇaḥ ।।

rayogaḥ syāt kiyān guṇaḥ rayogāt syāt kiyān guṇaḥ
nigūḍha-śalyāharaṇe śastra-kṣārāgni-karmaṇi ।
pīta-madyaś viṣahate sukhaṃ vaidya-vikatthanām ।।

śastra-kṣārāgni-karmasu
analottejanaṃ rucyaṃ śoka-śrama-vinodakam ।
na cātaḥ param asty anyad ārogya-bala-puṣṭi-kṛt ।।

śoka-śrama-vinodanam
rakṣatā jīvitaṃ tasmāt peyam ātma-vatā sadā ।
āśritopāśrita-hitaṃ paramaṃ dharma-sādhanam ।।

snātaḥ praṇamya sura-vipra-gurūn yathā-svaṃ vṛttiṃ vidhāya ca samasta-parigrahasya ।
āpāna-bhūmim atha gandha-jalābhiṣiktām āhāra-maṇḍapa-samīpa-gatāṃ śrayet ।।

sv-āstṛte atha śayane kamanīye mitra-bhṛtya-ramaṇī-samavetaḥ ।
svaṃ yaśaḥ kathaka-cāraṇa-saṃghair uddhataṃ niśamayann ati-lokam ।।

vilāsinīnāṃ ca vilāsa-śobhi gītaṃ sa-nṛtyaṃ kala-tūrya-ghoṣaiḥ ।
kāñcī-kalāpaiś cala-kiṅkiṇīkaiḥ krīḍā-vihaṅgaiś ca kṛtānunādam ।।

ītaṃ sa-nṛttaṃ kala-tūrya-ghoṣaiḥ āñcī-kalāpaiḥ
sphuṭa-kiṅkiṇīkaiḥ
maṇi-kanaka-samutthair āvaneyair vicitraiḥ ।।

aṇi-kanaka-samutthair aupageyair vicitraiḥ v
maṇi-kanaka-samutthaiḥ pāna-pātrair vicitraiḥ
sa-jala-vividha-lekha-kṣauma-vastrāvṛtāṅgaiḥ ।।

a-jala-vividha-bhakti-kṣauma-vastrāvṛtāṅgaiḥ api muni-jana-citta-kṣobha-saṃpādinībhiś ।।
cakita-hariṇa-lola-prekṣaṇībhiḥ priyābhiḥ ।।
akita-hariṇa-lola-prekṣaṇābhiḥ priyābhiḥ
stana-nitamba-kṛtād ati-gauravād alasam ākulam īśvara-saṃbhramāt ।
iti gataṃ dadhatībhir a-saṃsthitaṃ taruṇa-citta-vilobhana-kārmaṇam ।।

yauvanāsava-mattābhir vilāsādhiṣṭhitātmabhiḥ ।
saṃcāryamāṇaṃ yuga-pat tanv-aṅgībhir itas-tataḥ ।।

tāla-vṛnta-nalinī-dalānilaiḥ śītalī-kṛtam atīva śītalaiḥ ।
darśane api vidadhad vaśānugam svāditaṃ kim uta citta-janmanaḥ ।।

evitaṃ kim uta citta-janmanaḥ
cūta-rasendu-mṛgaiḥ kṛta-vāsaṃ mallikayojjvalayā ca sa-nātham ।
sphāṭika-śukti-gataṃ sa-taraṅgaṃ kāntam an-aṅgam ivodvahad aṅgam ।।

allikayojjvalayātha sa-nātham phāṭika-śukti-gataṃ su-taraṅgaṃ
tālīśādyaṃ cūrṇam elādikaṃ vā hṛdyaṃ prāśya prāg vayaḥ-sthāpanaṃ vā ।
tat-prārthibhyo bhūmi-bhāge su-mṛṣṭe toyonmiśraṃ dāpayitvā tataś ca ।।

ṛdyaṃ prāśyaṃ prāg vayaḥ-sthāpanaṃ vā
dhṛti-mān smṛti-mān nityam an-ūnādhikam ācaran ।
ucitenopacāreṇa sarvam evopapādayan ।।

-nyūnādhikam ācaran ditenopacāreṇa arvam 
evopapālayan
jita-vikasitāsita-saro-ja-nayana-saṃkrānti-vardhita-śrīkam ।
kāntā-mukham iva saurabha-hṛta-madhu-pa-gaṇaṃ piben madyam ।।

-ja-nayana-saṃkrānta-vardhita-śrīkam -ja-nayanaṃ sat
kānti-vardhita-śrīkam
pītvaivaṃ caṣaka-dvayaṃ parijanaṃ san-mānya sarvaṃ tato ।।

ītvaivaṃ caṣaka-trayaṃ parijanaṃ san-mānya sarvaṃ tato
ītvaivaṃ caṣaka-dvayaṃ parijanaṃ saṃbhāvya sarvaṃ tato
gatvāhāra-bhuvaṃ puraḥ su-bhiṣajo bhuñjīta bhūyo atra ca ।।
māṃsāpūpa-ghṛtārdrakādi-haritair yuktaṃ sa-sauvarcalair ।।dvis trir vā niśi cālpam eva vanitā-saṃvalganārthaṃ pibet ।।rahasi dayitām aṅke kṛtvā bhujāntara-pīḍanāt ।।pulakita-tanuṃ jāta-svedāṃ sa-kampa-payo-dharām ।।yadi sa-rabhasaṃ sīdhor vāraṃ na pāyayate kṛtī ।।
adi sa-rabhasaṃ sīdhūdgāraṃ na pāyayate kṛtī kim anubhavati kleśa-prāyaṃ tato gṛha-tantra-tām ।।

im anubhavati kleśa-prāyāṃ vṛthā gṛha-tantra-tām
im anubhavati kleśa-prāyāṃ tadā gṛha-tantra-tām
vara-tanu-vaktra-saṃgati-su-gandhi-taraṃ sarakam ।।
drutam iva padma-rāga-maṇim āsava-rūpa-dharam ।।bhavati rati-śrameṇa ca madaḥ pibato alpam api ।।kṣayam ata ojasaḥ pariharan sa śayīta param ।।
itthaṃ yuktyā piban madyaṃ na tri-vargād vihīyate ।
a-sāra-saṃsāra-sukhaṃ paramaṃ cādhigacchati ।।

aiśvaryasyopabhogo ayaṃ spṛhaṇīyaḥ surair api ।
anya-thā hi vipatsu syāt paścāt tāpendhanaṃ dhanam ।।

nya-thā hi vipatsv asya
upabhogena rahito bhoga-vān iti nindyate ।
nirmito ati-kad-aryo ayaṃ vidhinā nidhi-pālakaḥ ।।

tasmād vyavasthayā pānaṃ pānasya satataṃ hitam ।
jitvā viṣaya-lubdhānām indriyāṇāṃ sva-tantra-tām ।।

asmād avasthayā pānaṃ
vidhir vasu-matām eṣa bhaviṣyad-vasavas tu ye ।
yathopapatti tair madyaṃ pātavyaṃ mātrayā hitam ।।

yāvad dṛṣṭer na saṃbhrāntir yāvan na kṣobhate manaḥ ।
tāvad eva virantavyaṃ madyād ātma-vatā sadā ।।

abhyaṅgodvartana-snāna-vāsa-dhūpānulepanaiḥ ।
snigdhoṣṇair bhāvitaś cānnaiḥ pānaṃ vātottaraḥ pibet ।।

śītopacārair vividhair madhura-snigdha-śītalaiḥ ।
paittiko bhāvitaś cānnaiḥ piban madyaṃ na sīdati ।।

upacārair a-śiśirair yava-godhūma-bhuk pibet ।
ślaiṣmiko dhanva-jair māṃsair madyaṃ māricikaiḥ saha ।।

ślaiṣmiko jāṅgalair māṃsair adyaṃ maricakaiḥ saha
tatra vāte hitaṃ madyaṃ prāyaḥ paiṣṭika-gauḍikam ।
pitte sāmbho madhu kaphe mārdvīkāriṣṭa-mādhavam ।।

ādhvīkāriṣṭa-mādhavam
prāk pibec chlaiṣmiko madyaṃ bhuktasyopari paittikaḥ ।
vātikas tu piben madhye sama-doṣo yathecchayā ।।

ama-doṣo yathecchati ama-doṣo yad-ṛcchayā
madeṣu vāta-pitta-ghnaṃ prāyo mūrchāsu ceṣyate ।
sarva-trāpi viśeṣeṇa pittam evopalakṣayet ।।

śītāḥ pradehā maṇayaḥ sekā vyajana-mārutāḥ ।
sitā drākṣekṣu-kharjūra-kāśmarya-sva-rasāḥ payaḥ ।।

siddhaṃ madhura-vargeṇa rasā yūṣāḥ sa-dāḍimāḥ ।
ṣaṣṭikāḥ śālayo raktā yavāḥ sarpiś ca jīvanam ।।

kalyāṇakaṃ mahā-tiktaṃ ṣaṭ-palaṃ payasāgnikaḥ ।
pippalyo vā śilāhvaṃ vā rasāyana-vidhānataḥ ।।

tri-phalā vā prayoktavyā sa-ghṛta-kṣaudra-śarkarā ।
prasakta-vegeṣu hitaṃ mukha-nāsāvarodhanam ।।

pibed vā mānuṣī-kṣīraṃ tena dadyāc ca nāvanam ।
mṛṇāla-bisa-kṛṣṇā vā lihyāt kṣaudreṇa sābhayāḥ ।।

ibed vā mānuṣaṃ kṣīraṃ
durālabhāṃ vā mustaṃ vā śītena salilena vā ।
piben marica-kolāsthi-majjośīrāhikesaram ।।

dhātrī-phala-rase siddhaṃ pathyā-kvāthena vā ghṛtam ।
kuryāt kriyāṃ yathoktāṃ ca yathā-doṣa-balodayam ।।

pañca karmāṇi ceṣṭāni secanaṃ śoṇitasya ca ।
sat-tvasyālambanaṃ jñānam a-gṛddhir viṣayeṣu ca ।।

madeṣv ati-pravṛddheṣu mūrchāyeṣu ca yojayet ।
tīkṣṇaṃ saṃnyāsa-vihitaṃ viṣa-ghnaṃ viṣa-jeṣu ca ।।

arma saṃnyāsa-vihitaṃ iṣa-ghnaṃ viṣa-jeṣu tu
āśu prayojyaṃ saṃnyāse su-tīkṣṇaṃ nasyam añjanam ।
dhūmaḥ pradhamanaṃ todaḥ sūcībhiś ca nakhāntare ।।

hūmaṃ pradhamanaṃ todaḥ ūcībhiś ca nakhāntaraiḥ
keśānāṃ luñcanaṃ dāho daṃśo daśana-vṛścikaiḥ ।
kaṭv-amla-gālanaṃ vaktre kapikacchv-avagharṣaṇam ।।

apikacchvāvagharṣaṇam
utthito labdha-saṃjñaś ca laśuna-sva-rasaṃ pibet ।
khādet sa-vyoṣa-lavaṇaṃ bījapūraka-kesaram ।।

laghv-anna-prati tīkṣṇoṣṇam adyāt sroto-viśuddhaye ।
vismāpanaiḥ saṃsmaraṇaiḥ priya-śravaṇa-darśanaiḥ ।।

aghv annaṃ kaṭu-tīkṣṇoṣṇam
paṭubhir gīta-vāditra-śabdair vyāyāma-śīlanaiḥ ।
sraṃsanollekhanair dhūmaiḥ śoṇitasyāvasecanaiḥ ।।

upācaret taṃ pratatam anubandha-bhayāt punaḥ ।
tasya saṃrakṣitavyaṃ ca manaḥ pralaya-hetutaḥ ।।

cikitsāsthāna
kāle sādhāraṇe vy-abhre nāti-dur-balam arśasam ।
viśuddha-koṣṭhaṃ laghv-alpam anulomanam āśitam ।।

iśuddha-koṣṭhaṃ laghv-annam
śuciṃ kṛta-svasty-ayanaṃ mukta-viṇ-mūtram a-vyatham ।
śayane phalake vānya-narotsaṅge vyapāśritam ।।

pūrveṇa kāyenottānaṃ praty-āditya-gudaṃ samam ।
samunnata-kaṭī-deśam atha yantraṇa-vāsasā ।।

sakthnoḥ śiro-dharāyāṃ ca parikṣiptam ṛju sthitam ।
ālambitaṃ paricaraiḥ sarpiṣābhyakta-pāyave ।।

tato asmai sarpiṣābhyaktaṃ nidadhyād ṛju yantrakam ।
śanair anu-sukhaṃ pāyau tato dṛṣṭvā pravāhaṇāt ।।

yantre praviṣṭaṃ dur-nāma plota-guṇṭhitayānu ca ।
śalākayotpīḍya bhiṣag yathokta-vidhinā dahet ।।

antre praviṣṭe dur-nāma
kṣāreṇaivārdram itarat kṣāreṇa jvalanena vā ।
mahad vā balinaś chittvā vīta-yantram athāturam ।।

sv-abhyakta-pāyu-jaghanam avagāhe nidhāpayet ।
nir-vāta-mandira-sthasya tato asyācāram ādiśet ।।

ir-vātāgāra-saṃsthasya
ekaikam iti saptāhāt saptāhāt samupācaret ।
prāg dakṣiṇaṃ tato vāmam arśaḥ pṛṣṭhāgra-jaṃ tataḥ ।।

bahv-arśasaḥ su-dagdhasya syād vāyor anuloma-tā ।
rucir anne agni-paṭu-tā svāsthyaṃ varṇa-balodayaḥ ।।

vasti-śūle tv adho nābher lepayec chlakṣṇa-kalkitaiḥ ।
varṣābhū-kuṣṭha-surabhi-miśi-lohāmarāhvayaiḥ ।।

śakṛn-mūtra-pratīghāte pariṣekāvagāhayoḥ ।
varaṇālambuṣair aṇḍa-gokaṇṭaka-punarnavaiḥ ।।

śakṛn-mūtra-parīghāte
suṣavī-surabhībhyāṃ ca kvātham uṣṇaṃ prayojayet ।
sa-sneham atha-vā kṣīraṃ tailaṃ vā vāta-nāśanam ।।

yuñjītānnaṃ śakṛd-bhedi snehān vāta-ghna-dīpanān ।
athā-prayojya-dāhasya nirgatān kapha-vāta-jān ।।

sa-stambha-kaṇḍū-ruk-śophān abhyajya guda-kīlakān ।
bilva-mūlāgnika-kṣāra-kuṣṭhaiḥ siddhena secayet ।।

aṃrambha-kaṇḍū-ruk-śophān aṃstambha-kaṇḍū-ruk-śophān
tailenāhi-biḍāloṣṭra-varāha-vasayātha-vā ।
svedayed anu piṇḍena drava-svedena vā punaḥ ।।

kāsīsaṃ saindhavaṃ rāsnā śuṇṭhī kuṣṭhaṃ ca lāṅgalī ।
śilābhrakāśvamāraṃ ca jantuhṛd danti-citrakau ।।

haritālaṃ tathā svarṇakṣīrī taiś ca pacet samaiḥ ।
tailaṃ sudhārka-payasī gavāṃ mūtre catur-guṇe ।।

etad abhyaṅgato arśāṃsi kṣāra-vat pātayed drutam ।
kṣāra-karma-karaṃ hy etan na ca dūṣayate valīm ।।

saktūnāṃ piṇḍikābhir vā snigdhānāṃ taila-sarpiṣā ।
rāsnāyā hapuṣāyā vā piṇḍair vā kārṣṇyagandhikaiḥ ।।

iṇḍair vā kārṣakānvitaiḥ
arka-mūlaṃ śamī-pattram nṛ-keśaḥ sarpa-kañcukam ।
mārjāra-carma sarpiś ca dhūpanaṃ hitam arśasām ।।

tathāśvagandhā surasā bṛhatī pippalī ghṛtam ।
dhānyāmla-piṣṭair jīmūta-bījais taj-jālakaṃ mṛdu ।।

lepitaṃ chāyayā śuṣkaṃ vartir guda-ja-śātanī ।
sa-jāla-mūla-jīmūta-lehe vā kṣāra-saṃyute ।।

guñjā-sūraṇa-kūṣmāṇḍa-bījair vartis tathā-guṇā ।
snuk-kṣīrārdra-niśā-lepas tathā go-mūtra-kalkitaiḥ ।।

kṛkavāku-śakṛt-kṛṣṇā-niśā-guñjā-phalais tathā ।
snuk-kṣīra-piṣṭaiḥ ṣaḍgranthā-halinī-vāraṇāsthibhiḥ ।।

kulīraśṛṅgī-vijayā-kuṣṭhāruṣkara-tutthakaiḥ ।
śigru-mūlaka-jair bījaiḥ pattrair aśvaghna-nimba-jaiḥ ।।

śigru-mūlaka-bījair vā
pīlu-mūlena bilvena hiṅgunā ca samanvitaiḥ ।
kuṣṭhaṃ śirīṣa-bījāni pippalyaḥ saindhavaṃ guḍaḥ ।।

arka-kṣīraṃ sudhā-kṣīraṃ tri-phalā ca pralepanam ।
ārkaṃ payaḥ sudhā-kāṇḍaṃ kaṭukālābu-pallavāḥ ।।

ārkaṃ payaḥ snuhī-kāṇḍaṃ
karañjo basta-mūtraṃ ca lepanaṃ śreṣṭham arśasām ।
ānuvāsanikair lepaḥ pippaly-ādyaiś ca pūjitaḥ ।।

ebhir evauṣadhaiḥ kuryāt tailāny abhyañjanāya ca ।
dhūpanālepanābhyaṅgaiḥ prasravanti gudāṅkurāḥ ।।

bhir lepauṣadhaiḥ kuryāt ailāny abhyañjanāni ca
saṃcitaṃ duṣṭa-rudhiraṃ tataḥ saṃpadyate sukhī ।
a-vartamānam ucchūna-kaṭhinebhyo hared asṛk ।।

arśobhyo jala-jā-śastra-sūcī-kūrcaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
śītoṣṇa-snigdha-rūkṣair hi na vyādhir upaśāmyati ।।

śītoṣṇa-snigdha-rūkṣādyair
rakte duṣṭe bhiṣak tasmād raktam evāvasecayet ।
yo jāto go-rasaḥ kṣīrād vahni-cūrṇāvacūrṇitāt ।।

ahu-mūlāvacūrṇitāt
pibaṃs tam eva tenaiva bhuñjāno guda-jān jayet ।
kovidārasya mūlānāṃ mathitena rajaḥ piban ।।

athitena rajaḥ pibet
aśnan jīrṇe ca pathyāni mucyate hata-nāmabhiḥ ।
guda-śvayathu-śūlārto mandāgnir gaulmikān pibet ।।

hiṅgv-ādīn anu-takraṃ vā khāded guḍa-harītakīm ।
takreṇa vā pibet pathyā-vellāgni-kuṭaja-tvacaḥ ।।

iṅgv-ādīn anu-takrāṃ vā akreṇa vā pibet pathyāṃ 
vellāgni-kuṭaja-tvacaḥ
kaliṅga-magadhā-jyotiḥ-sūraṇān vāṃśa-vardhitān ।
koṣṇāmbunā vā tri-paṭu-vyoṣa-hiṅgv-amla-vetasam ।।

yuktaṃ bilva-kapitthābhyāṃ mahauṣadha-viḍena vā ।
aruṣkarair yavānyā vā pradadyāt takra-tarpaṇam ।।

āruṣkarair yavānyā vā
dadyād vā hapuṣā-hiṅgu-citrakaṃ takra-saṃyutam ।
māsaṃ takrānu-pānāni khādet pīlu-phalāni vā ।।

pibed ahar ahas takraṃ nir-anno vā pra-kāmataḥ ।
aty-arthaṃ manda-kāyāgnes takram evāvacārayet ।।

ty-artha-manda-kāyāgnes
saptāhaṃ vā daśāhaṃ vā māsārdhaṃ māsam eva ca ।
bala-kāla-vikāra-jño bhiṣak takraṃ prayojayet ।।

sāyaṃ vā lāja-saktūnāṃ dadyāt takrāvalehikām ।
jīrṇe takre pradadyād vā takra-peyāṃ sa-saindhavām ।।

takrānu-pānaṃ sa-snehaṃ takraudanam ataḥ param ।
yūṣai rasair vā takrāḍhyaiḥ śālīn bhuñjīta mātrayā ।।

rūkṣam ardhoddhṛta-snehaṃ yataś cān-uddhṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।
takraṃ doṣāgni-bala-vit tri-vidhaṃ tat prayojyet ।।

na virohanti guda-jāḥ punas takra-samāhatāḥ ।
niṣiktaṃ tad dhi dahati bhūmāv api tṛṇolupam ।।

iṣiktaṃ tad vidahati
srotaḥsu takra-śuddheṣu raso dhātūn upaiti yaḥ ।
tena puṣṭir balaṃ varṇaḥ paraṃ tuṣṭiś ca jāyate ।।

vāta-śleṣma-vikārāṇāṃ śataṃ ca vinivartate ।
mathitaṃ bhājane kṣudra-bṛhatī-phala-lepite ।।

niśāṃ paryuṣitaṃ peyam icchadbhir guda-ja-kṣayam ।
dhānyopakuñcikājājī-hapuṣā-pippalī-dvayaiḥ ।।

kāravī-granthika-śaṭhī-yavāny-agni-yavānakaiḥ ।
cūrṇitair ghṛta-pātra-sthaṃ nāty-amlaṃ takram āsutam ।।

-yavāny-agni-yavānikaiḥ
takrāriṣṭaṃ pibej jātaṃ vyaktāmla-kaṭu kāmataḥ ।
dīpanaṃ rocanaṃ varṇyaṃ kapha-vātānulomanam ।।

guda-śvayathu-kaṇḍv-arti-nāśanaṃ bala-vardhanam ।
tvacaṃ citraka-mūlasya piṣṭvā kumbhaṃ pralepayet ।।

takraṃ vā dadhi vā tatra jātam arśo-haraṃ pibet ।
bhārgy-āsphotāmṛtā-pañca-koleṣv apy eṣa saṃvidhiḥ ।।

piṣṭair gaja-kaṇā-pāṭhā-kāravī-pañca-kolakaiḥ ।
tumburv-ajājī-dhanikā-bilva-madhyaiś ca kalpayet ।।

phalāmlān yamaka-snehān peyā-yūṣa-rasādikān ।
ebhir evauṣadhaiḥ sādhyaṃ vāri sarpiś ca dīpanam ।।

kramo ayaṃ bhinna-śakṛtāṃ vakṣyate gāḍha-varcasām ।
snehāḍhyaiḥ saktubhir yuktāṃ lavaṇāṃ vāruṇīṃ pibet ।।

lavaṇā eva vā takra-sīdhu-dhānyāmla-vāruṇīḥ ।
prāg-bhaktān yamake bhṛṣṭān saktubhiś cāvacūrṇitān ।।

rāg-bhaktaṃ yamake bhṛṣṭān
karañja-pallavān khāded vāta-varco-'nulomanān ।
sa-guḍaṃ nāgaraṃ pāṭhāṃ guḍa-kṣāra-ghṛtāni vā ।।

a-guḍaṃ nāgaraṃ pāṭhā- -guḍa-kṣāra-ghṛtāni vā
go-mūtrādhyuṣitām adyāt sa-guḍāṃ vā harītakīm ।
pathyā-śata-dvayān mūtra-droṇenā-mūtra-saṃkṣayāt ।।

athyā-śata-dvayaṃ mūtra-
pakvāt khādet sa-madhunī dve dve hanti kaphodbhavān ।
dur-nāma-kuṣṭha-śvayathu-gulma-mehodara-kṛmīn ।।

aktvā khādet sa-madhunī
granthy-arbudāpacī-sthaulya-pāṇḍu-rogāḍhya-mārutān ।
ajaśṛṅgī-jaṭā-kalkam ajā-mūtreṇa yaḥ pibet ।।

guḍa-vārtāka-bhuk tasya naśyanty āśu gudāṅkurāḥ ।
śreṣṭhā-rasena trivṛtāṃ pathyāṃ takreṇa vā saha ।।

pathyāṃ vā pippalī-yuktāṃ ghṛta-bhṛṣṭāṃ guḍānvitām ।
atha-vā sa-trivṛd-dantīṃ bhakṣayed anulomanīm ।।

hate gudāśraye doṣe guda-jā yānti saṃkṣayam ।
dāḍima-sva-rasājājī-yavānī-guḍa-nāgaraiḥ ।।

ṛte gudāśraye doṣe
pāṭhayā vā yutaṃ takraṃ vāta-varco-'nulomanam ।
sīdhuṃ vā gauḍam atha-vā sa-citraka-mahauṣadham ।।

pibet surāṃ vā hapuṣā-pāṭhā-sauvarcalānvitām ।
daśādi-daśakair vṛddhāḥ pippalīr dvi-picuṃ tilān ।।

ippalīr dvi-picuṃ tilāt
pītvā kṣīreṇa labhate balaṃ deha-hutāśayoḥ ।
duḥsparśakena bilvena yavānyā nāgareṇa vā ।।

avānyā nāgareṇa ca
ekaikenāpi saṃyuktā pāṭhā hanty arśasāṃ rujam ।
salilasya vahe paktvā prasthārdham abhayā-tvacām ।।

rasthārdham abhayā-tvacam
prasthaṃ dhātryā daśa-palaṃ kapitthānāṃ tato ardhataḥ ।
viśālāṃ lodhra-marica-kṛṣṇā-vellailavālukam ।।

dvi-palāṃśaṃ pṛthak pāda-śeṣe pūte guḍāt tule ।
dattvā prasthaṃ ca dhātakyāḥ sthāpayed ghṛta-bhājane ।।

attvā prasthaṃ tu dhātakyāḥ
pakṣāt sa śīlito ariṣṭaḥ karoty agniṃ nihanti ca ।
guda-ja-grahaṇī-pāṇḍu-kuṣṭhodara-gara-jvarān ।।

śvayathu-plīha-hṛd-roga-gulma-yakṣma-vami-kṛmīn ।
jala-droṇe paced dantī-daśa-mūla-varāgnikān ।।

pālikān pāda-śeṣe tu kṣiped guḍa-tulāṃ param ।
pūrva-vat sarvam asya syād ānulomi-taras tv ayam ।।

paced durālabhā-prasthaṃ droṇe apāṃ prāsṛtaiḥ saha ।
dantī-pāṭhāgni-vijayā-vāsāmalaka-nāgaraiḥ ।।

roṇe apāṃ dvi-palaiḥ saha
tasmin sitā-śataṃ dadyāt pāda-sthe anyac ca pūrva-vat ।
limpet kumbhaṃ tu phalinī-kṛṣṇā-cavyājya-mākṣikaiḥ ।।

prāg-bhaktam ānulomyāya phalāmlaṃ vā pibed ghṛtam ।
cavya-citraka-siddhaṃ vā yava-kṣāra-guḍānvitam ।।

pippalī-mūla-siddhaṃ vā sa-guḍa-kṣāra-nāgaram ।
pippalī-pippalī-mūla-dhānakā-dāḍimair ghṛtam ।।

-dhānyakā-dāḍimair ghṛtam
dadhnā ca sādhitaṃ vāta-śakṛn-mūtra-vibandha-nut ।
palāśa-kṣāra-toyena tri-guṇena paced ghṛtam ।।

-śakṛn-mūtra-vibandha-hṛt
vatsakādi-pratīvāpam arśo-ghnaṃ dīpanaṃ param ।
pañca-kolābhayā-kṣāra-yavānī-viḍa-saindhavaiḥ ।।

sa-pāṭhā-dhānya-maricaiḥ sa-bilvair dadhi-mat ghṛtam ।
sādhayet taj jayaty āśu guda-vaṅkṣaṇa-vedanām ।।

pravāhikāṃ guda-bhraṃśaṃ mūtra-kṛcchraṃ parisravam ।
pāṭhājamoda-dhanikā-śvadaṃṣṭrā-pañca-kolakaiḥ ।।

sa-bilvair dadhni cāṅgerī-sva-rase ca catur-guṇe ।
hanty ājyaṃ siddham ānāhaṃ mūtra-kṛcchraṃ pravāhikām ।।

guda-bhraṃśārti-guda-ja-grahaṇī-gada-mārutān ।
śikhi-tittiri-lāvānāṃ rasān amlān su-saṃskṛtān ।।

dakṣāṇāṃ vartakānāṃ vā dadyād viḍ-vāta-saṃgrahe ।
vāstukāgni-trivṛd-dantī-pāṭhāmlīkādi-pallavān ।।

anyac ca kapha-vāta-ghnaṃ śākaṃ ca laghu bhedi ca ।
sa-hiṅgu yamake bhṛṣṭaṃ siddhaṃ dadhi-saraiḥ saha ।।

iddhaṃ dadhi-sareṇa ca
dhanikā-pañca-kolābhyāṃ piṣṭābhyāṃ dāḍimāmbunā ।
ārdrikāyāḥ kisalayaiḥ śakalair ārdrakasya ca ।।

yuktam aṅgāra-dhūpena hṛdyena surabhī-kṛtam ।
sa-jīrakaṃ sa-maricaṃ viḍa-sauvarcalotkaṭam ।।

uktam aṅgāra-dhūmena
vātottarasya rūkṣasya mandāgner baddha-varcasaḥ ।
kalpayed rakta-śāly-anna-vyañjanaṃ śāka-vad rasān ।।

alpayed rakta-śāly-annaṃ yañjanaṃ śāka-vad rasān 
vyañjanāñ chāka-vad rasān
go-godhā-chagaloṣṭrāṇāṃ viśeṣāt kravya-bhojinām ।
madirāṃ śārkaraṃ gauḍaṃ sīdhuṃ takraṃ tuṣodakam ।।

ariṣṭaṃ mastu pānīyaṃ pānīyaṃ vālpakaṃ śṛtam ।
dhānyena dhānya-śuṇṭhībhyāṃ kaṇṭakārikayātha-vā ।।

ante bhaktasya madhye vā vāta-varco-'nulomanam ।
viḍ-vāta-kapha-pittānām ānulomye hi nir-male ।।

gude śāmyanti guda-jāḥ pāvakaś cābhivardhate ।
udāvarta-parītā ye ye cāty-arthaṃ virūkṣitāḥ ।।

viloma-vātāḥ śūlārtās teṣv iṣṭam anuvāsanam ।
pippalīṃ madanaṃ bilvaṃ śatāhvāṃ madhukaṃ vacām ।।

kuṣṭhaṃ śaṭhīṃ puṣkarākhyaṃ citrakaṃ devadāru ca ।
piṣṭvā tailaṃ vipaktavyaṃ dvi-guṇa-kṣīra-saṃyutam ।।

uṣṭhaṃ śaṭhīṃ puṣkarāhvaṃ uṣṭhaṃ śaṭhīṃ pauṣkarākhyaṃ 
uṣṭhaṃ śuṇṭhīṃ puṣkarākhyaṃ
arśasāṃ mūḍha-vātānāṃ tac chreṣṭham anuvāsanam ।
guda-niḥsaraṇaṃ śūlaṃ mūtra-kṛcchraṃ pravāhikām ।।

kaṭy-ūru-pṛṣṭha-daurbalyam ānāhaṃ vaṅkṣaṇāśrayam ।
picchā-srāvaṃ gude śophaṃ vāta-varco-vinigraham ।।

utthānaṃ bahu-śo yac ca jayet tac cānuvāsanāt ।
nirūhaṃ vā prayuñjīta sa-kṣīraṃ pāñcamūlikam ।।

sa-mūtra-sneha-lavaṇaṃ kalkair yuktaṃ phalādibhiḥ ।
atha raktārśasāṃ vīkṣya mārutasya kaphasya vā ।।

ārutasya kaphasya ca
anubandhaṃ tataḥ snigdhaṃ rūkṣaṃ vā yojayed dhimam ।
śakṛc chyāvaṃ kharaṃ rūkṣam adho niryāti nānilaḥ ।।

kaṭy-ūru-guda-śūlaṃ ca hetur yadi ca rūkṣaṇam ।
tatrānubandho vātasya śleṣmaṇo yadi viṭ ślathā ।।

śvetā pītā guruḥ snigdhā sa-picchaḥ stimito gudaḥ ।
hetuḥ snigdha-gurur vidyād yathā-svaṃ cāsra-lakṣaṇāt ।।

duṣṭe asre śodhanaṃ kāryaṃ laṅghanaṃ ca yathā-balam ।
yāvac ca doṣaiḥ kāluṣyaṃ srutes tāvad upekṣaṇam ।।

doṣāṇāṃ pācanārthaṃ ca vahni-saṃdhukṣaṇāya ca ।
saṃgrahāya ca raktasya paraṃ tiktair upācaret ।।

yat tu prakṣīṇa-doṣasya raktaṃ vātolbaṇasya vā ।
snehais tat sādhayet yuktaiḥ pānābhyañjana-vastiṣu ।।

yat tu pittolbaṇaṃ raktaṃ gharma-kāle pravartate ।
stambhanīyaṃ tad ekāntān na ced vāta-kaphānugam ।।

sa-kaphe asre pibet pākyaṃ śuṇṭhī-kuṭaja-valkalam ।
kirātatiktakaṃ śuṇṭhīṃ dhanvayāsaṃ ku-candanam ।।

dārvī-tvaṅ-nimba-sevyāni tvacaṃ vā dāḍimodbhavām ।
kuṭaja-tvak-phalaṃ tārkṣyaṃ mākṣikaṃ ghuṇavallabhām ।।

pibet taṇḍula-toyena kalkitaṃ vā mayūrakam ।
tulāṃ divyāmbhasi paced ārdrāyāḥ kuṭaja-tvacaḥ ।।

nī-rasāyāṃ tvaci kvāthe dadyāt sūkṣma-rajī-kṛtān ।
samaṅgā-phalinī-moca-rasān muṣṭy-aṃśakān samān ।।

taiś ca śakrayavān pūte tato darvī-pralepanam ।
paktvāvalehaṃ līḍhvā ca taṃ yathāgni-balaṃ pibet ।।

aiś ca śakrayavān pūtaṃ
peyāṃ maṇḍaṃ payaś chāgaṃ gavyaṃ vā chāga-dugdha-bhuk ।
leho ayaṃ śamayaty āśu raktātīsāra-pāyu-jān ।।

bala-vad rakta-pittaṃ ca sravad ūrdhvam adho api vā ।
kuṭaja-tvak-tulāṃ droṇe paced aṣṭāṃśa-śeṣitam ।।

aced aṣṭāṃśa-śeṣitām
kalkī-kṛtya kṣipet tatra tārkṣya-śailaṃ kaṭu-trayam ।
lodhra-dvayaṃ moca-rasaṃ balāṃ dāḍima-jaṃ tvacam ।।

bilva-karkaṭikāṃ mustaṃ samaṅgāṃ dhātakī-phalam ।
palonmitaṃ daśa-palaṃ kuṭajasyaiva ca tvacaḥ ।।

triṃśat palāni guḍato ghṛtāt pūte ca viṃśatiḥ ।
tat pakvaṃ leha-tāṃ yātaṃ dhānye pakṣa-sthitaṃ lihan ।।

sarvārśo-grahaṇī-doṣa-śvāsa-kāsān niyacchati ।
lodhraṃ tilān moca-rasaṃ samaṅgāṃ candanotpalam ।।

-śvāsa-kāsān nibarhati
pāyayitvāja-dugdhena śālīṃs tenaiva bhojayet ।
yaṣṭy-āhva-padmakānantā-payasyā-kṣīra-moraṭam ।।

sa-sitā-madhu pātavyaṃ śīta-toyena tena vā ।
lodhra-kaṭvaṅga-kuṭaja-samaṅgā-śālmalī-tvacam ।।

-samaṅgā-śālmalī-tvacaḥ
hima-kesara-yaṣṭy-āhva-sevyaṃ vā taṇḍulāmbunā ।
yavānīndrayavāḥ pāṭḥā bilvaṃ śuṇṭhī rasāñjanam ।।

cūrṇaś cale hitaḥ śūle pravṛtte cāti-śoṇite ।
dugdhikā-kaṇṭakārībhyāṃ siddhaṃ sarpiḥ praśasyate ।।

atha-vā dhātakī-lodhra-kuṭaja-tvak-phalotpalaiḥ ।
sa-kesarair yava-kṣāra-dāḍima-sva-rasena vā ।।

śarkarāmbho-ja-kiñjalka-sahitaṃ saha vā tilaiḥ ।
abhyastaṃ rakta-guda-jān nava-nītaṃ niyacchati ।।

chāgāni nava-nītājya-kṣīra-māṃsāni jāṅgalaḥ ।
an-amlo vā kad-amla vā sa-vāstuka-raso rasaḥ ।।

rakta-śāliḥ saro dadhnaḥ ṣaṣṭikas taruṇī surā ।
taruṇaś ca surā-maṇḍaḥ śoṇitasyauṣadhaṃ param ।।

peyā-yūṣa-rasādyeṣu palāṇḍuḥ kevalo api vā ।
sa jayaty ulbaṇaṃ raktaṃ mārutaṃ ca prayojitaḥ ।।

vātolbaṇāni prāyeṇa bhavanty asre ati-niḥsṛte ।
arśāṃsi tasmād adhikaṃ taj-jaye yatnam ācaret ।।

dṛṣṭvāsra-pittaṃ prabalam a-balau ca kaphānilau ।
śītopacāraḥ kartavyaḥ sarva-thā tat-praśāntaye ।।

na ced evaṃ śamas tasya snigdhoṣṇais tarpayet tataḥ ।
rasaiḥ koṣṇaiś ca sarpirbhir avapīḍaka-yojitaiḥ ।।

adā caivaṃ śamo na syāt
secayet taṃ kavoṣṇaiś ca kāmaṃ taila-payo-ghṛtaiḥ ।
yavāsa-kuśa-kāśānāṃ mūlaṃ puṣpaṃ ca śālmaleḥ ।।

nyagrodhodumbarāśvattha-śuṅgāś ca dvi-palonmitāḥ ।
tri-prasthe salilasyaitat kṣīra-prasthe ca sādhayet ।।

kṣīra-śeṣe kaṣāye ca tasmin pūte vimiśrayet ।
kalkī-kṛtaṃ moca-rasaṃ samaṅgāṃ candanotpalam ।।

priyaṅguṃ kauṭajaṃ bījaṃ kamalasya ca kesaram ।
picchā-vastir ayaṃ siddhaḥ sa-ghṛta-kṣaudra-śarkaraḥ ।।

pravāhikā-guda-bhraṃśa-rakta-srāva-jvarāpahaḥ ।
yaṣṭy-āhva-puṇḍarīkeṇa tathā moca-rasādibhiḥ ।।

kṣīra-dvi-guṇitaḥ pakvo deyaḥ sneho anuvāsanam ।
madhukotpala-lodhrāmbu samaṅgā bilva-candanam ।।

cavikātiviṣā mustaṃ pāṭhā kṣāro yavāgra-jaḥ ।
dārvī-tvaṅ nāgaraṃ māṃsī citrako devadāru ca ।।

cāṅgerī-sva-rase sarpiḥ sādhitaṃ tais tri-doṣa-jit ।
arśo-'tīsāra-grahaṇī-pāṇḍu-roga-jvarā-rucau ।।

mūtra-kṛcchre guda-bhraṃśe vasty-ānāhe pravāhaṇe ।
picchā-srāve arśasāṃ śūle deyaṃ tat paramauṣadham ।।

vyatyāsān madhurāmlāni śītoṣṇāni ca yojayet ।
nityam agni-balāpekṣī jayaty arśaḥ-kṛtān gadān ।।

ayaty arśaḥ-kṛtāṃ rujam
udāvartārtam abhyajya tailaiḥ śīta-jvarāpahaiḥ ।
su-snigdhaiḥ svedayet piṇḍair vartim asmai gude tataḥ ।।

abhyaktāṃ tat-karāṅguṣṭha-saṃnibhām anulomanīm ।
dadyāc chyāmā-trivṛd-dantī-pippalī-nīlinī-phalaiḥ ।।

vicūrṇitair dvi-lavaṇair guḍa-go-mūtra-saṃyutaiḥ ।
tad-van māgadhikā-rāṭha-gṛha-dhūmaiḥ sa-sarṣapaiḥ ।।

uḍa-go-mūtra-pācitaiḥ
eteṣām eva vā cūrṇaṃ gude nāḍyā vinirdhamet ।
tad-vighāte su-tīkṣṇaṃ tu vastiṃ snigdhaṃ prapīḍayet ।।

ṛjū-kuryād guda-sirā-viṇ-mūtra-maruto asya saḥ ।
bhūyo anubandhe vāta-ghnair virecyaḥ sneha-recanaiḥ ।।

ṛjū-kuryād guda-śiro-
anuvāsyaś ca raukṣyād dhi saṅgo māruta-varcasoḥ ।
tri-paṭu-tri-kaṭu-śreṣṭhā-danty-aruṣkara-citrakam ।।

jarjaraṃ sneha-mūtrāktam antar-dhūmaṃ vipācayet ।
śarāva-saṃdhau mṛl-lipte kṣāraḥ kalyāṇakāhvayaḥ ।।

sa pītaḥ sarpiṣā yukto bhakte vā snigdha-bhojinā ।
udāvarta-vibandhārśo-gulma-pāṇḍūdara-kṛmīn ।।

mūtra-saṅgāśmarī-śopha-hṛd-roga-grahaṇī-gadān ।
meha-plīha-rujānāha-śvāsa-kāsāṃś ca nāśayet ।।
sarvaṃ ca kuryād yat proktam arśasāṃ gāḍha-varcasām ।।droṇe apāṃ pūti-valka-dvi-tulam atha pacet pāda-śeṣe ca tasmin ।।
roṇe apāṃ pūti-valkaṃ dvi-tulam atha pacet pāda-śeṣe ca tasmin deyāśītir guḍasya pratanuka-rajaso vyoṣato aṣṭau palāni ।।
etan māsena jātaṃ janayati paramām ūṣmaṇaḥ pakti-śaktiṃ ।।śuktaṃ kṛtvānulomyaṃ prajayati guda-ja-plīha-gulmodarāṇi ।।
pacet tulāṃ pūti-karañja-valkād dve mūlataś citraka-kaṇṭakāryoḥ ।
droṇa-traye api caraṇāvaśeṣe pūte śataṃ tatra guḍasya dadyāt ।।

palikaṃ ca su-cūrṇitaṃ tri-jāta-tri-kaṭu-granthika-dāḍimāśmabhedam ।
pura-puṣkara-mūla-dhānya-cavyaṃ hapuṣām ārdrakam amla-vetasaṃ ca ।।

śītī-bhūtaṃ kṣaudra-viṃśaty-upetam ārdra-drākṣā-bījapūrārdrakaiś ca ।
yuktaṃ kāmaṃ gaṇḍikābhis tathekṣoḥ sarpiḥ-pātre māsa-mātreṇa jātam ।।

cukraṃ krakacam ivedaṃ dur-nāmnāṃ vahni-dīpanaṃ paramam ।
pāṇḍu-garodara-gulma-plīhānāhāśma-kṛcchra-ghnam ।।
droṇaṃ pīlu-rasasya vastra-galitaṃ nyastaṃ havir-bhājane ।।yuñjīta dvi-palair madā-madhuphalā-kharjūra-dhātrī-phalaiḥ ।।pāṭhā-mādri-durālabhāmla-vidula-vyoṣa-tvag-elollakaiḥ ।।
āṭhā-mādri-durālabhāmla-vidula-vyoṣa-tvag-ellāllakaiḥ spṛkkā-kola-lavaṅga-vella-capalā-mūlāgnikaiḥ pālikaiḥ ।।

guḍa-pala-śata-yojitaṃ nivāte nihitam idaṃ prapibaṃś ca pakṣa-mātrāt ।
niśamayati gudāṅkurān sa-gulmān anala-balaṃ prabalaṃ karoti cāśu ।।

raśamayati gudāṅkurān sa-gulmān
ekaika-śo daśa-pale daśa-mūla-kumbha-pāṭhā-dvayārka-ghuṇavallabha-kaṭphalānām ।
dagdhe srute anu kalaśena jalena pakve pāda-sthite guḍa-tulāṃ pala-pañcakaṃ ca ।।

-pāṭhābhayārka-ghuṇavallabha-kaṭphalānām
dadyāt praty-ekaṃ vyoṣa-cavyābhayānāṃ vahner muṣṭī dve yava-kṣārataś ca ।
darvīm ālimpan hanti līḍho guḍo ayaṃ gulma-plīhārśaḥ-kuṣṭha-mehāgni-sādān ।।

toya-droṇe citraka-mūla-tulārdhaṃ sādhyaṃ yāvat pāda-dala-stham athedam ।
aṣṭau dattvā jīrṇa-guḍasya palāni kvāthyaṃ bhūyaḥ sāndra-tayā samam etat ।।

ādhyaṃ yāvat pāda-jala-stham apy idam
tri-kaṭuka-miśi-pathyā-kuṣṭha-mustā-varāṅga-kṛmiripu-dahanailā-cūrṇa-kīrṇo avalehaḥ ।
jayati guda-ja-kuṣṭha-plīha-gulmodarāṇi prabalayati hutāśaṃ śaśvad abhyasyamānaḥ ।।

।।

ayati guda-ja-yukta-plīha-gulmodarāṇi
guḍa-vyoṣa-varā-vella-tilāruṣkara-citrakaiḥ ।
arśāṃsi hanti guṭikā tvag-vikāraṃ ca śīlitā ।।

mṛl-liptaṃ sauraṇaṃ kandaṃ paktvāgnau puṭa-pāka-vat ।
adyāt sa-taila-lavaṇaṃ dur-nāma-vinivṛttaye ।।

marica-pippali-nāgara-citrakān krama-vivardhita-bhāga-samāhṛtān ।
śikhi-catur-guṇa-sūraṇa-yojitān kuru guḍena guḍān guda-ja-cchidaḥ ।।

cūrṇī-kṛtāḥ ṣo-ḍaśa sūraṇasya bhāgās tato ardhena ca citrakasya ।
mahauṣadhād dvau maricasya caiko guḍena dur-nāma-jayāya piṇḍī ।।

pathyā-nāgara-kṛṣṇā-karañja-vellāgnibhiḥ sitā-tulyaiḥ ।
vaḍabā-mukha iva jarayati bahu-gurv api bhojanaṃ cūrṇaḥ ।।

ahu-gurv api bhojanaṃ cūrṇam
kaliṅga-lāṅgalī-kṛṣṇā-vahny-apāmārga-taṇḍulaiḥ ।
bhūnimba-saindhava-guḍair guḍā guda-ja-nāśanāḥ ।।

lavaṇottama-vahni-kaliṅga-yavāṃś ciribilva-mahāpicumanda-yutān ।
piba sapta-dinaṃ mathitāluḍitān yadi marditum icchasi pāyu-ruhān ।।

iba sapta-dinaṃ mathitālulitān adi marditum icchasi 
pāyu-ruhaḥ
śuṣkeṣu bhallātakam agryam uktaṃ bhaiṣajyam ārdreṣu tu vatsaka-tvak ।
sarveṣu sarvartuṣu kālaśeyam arśaḥsu balyaṃ ca malāpahaṃ ca ।।

bhittvā vibandhān anulomanāya yan mārutasyāgni-balāya yac ca ।
tad anna-pānauṣadham arśasena sevyaṃ vivarjyaṃ viparītam asmāt ।।

arśo-'tisāra-grahaṇī-vikārāḥ prāyeṇa cānyo-'nya-nidāna-bhūtāḥ ।
sanne anale santi na santi dīpte rakṣed atas teṣu viśeṣato agnim ।।

akṣet tatas teṣu viśeṣato agnim

cikitsāsthāna
atīsāro hi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ bhavaty āmāśayānvayaḥ ।
hatvāgniṃ vāta-je apy asmāt prāk tasmiō̃ laṅghanaṃ hitam ।।

rāg asmiō̃ laṅghanaṃ hitam
śūlānāha-prasekārtaṃ vāmayed atisāriṇam ।
doṣāḥ saṃnicitā ye ca vidagdhāhāra-mūrchitāḥ ।।

atīsārāya kalpante teṣūpekṣaiva bheṣajam ।
bhṛśotkleśa-pravṛtteṣu svayam eva calātmasu ।।

na tu saṃgrahaṇaṃ yojyaṃ pūrvam āmātisāriṇi ।
api cādhmāna-guru-tā-śūla-staimitya-kāriṇi ।।

rayojyaṃ na tu saṃgrāhi ūrvam āmolbaṇe na tu
prāṇadā prāṇa-dā doṣe vibaddhe saṃpravartinī ।
pibet prakvathitās toye madhya-doṣo viśoṣayan ।।

bhūtika-pippalī-śuṇṭhī-vacā-dhānya-harītakīḥ ।
atha-vā bilva-dhanikā-musta-nāgara-vālakam ।।

viḍa-pāṭhā-vacā-pathyā-kṛmijin-nāgarāṇi vā ।
śuṇṭhī-ghana-vacā-mādrī-bilva-vatsaka-hiṅgu vā ।।

śasyate tv alpa-doṣāṇām upavāso atisāriṇām ।
vacā-prativiṣābhyāṃ vā mustā-parpaṭakena vā ।।

hrīvera-nāgarābhyāṃ vā vipakvaṃ pāyayej jalam ।
yukte anna-kāle kṣut-kṣāmaṃ laghv-anna-prati bhojayet ।।

aghv annaṃ pratibhojayet
tathā sa śīghraṃ prāpnoti rucim agni-balaṃ balam ।
takreṇāvanti-somena yavāgvā tarpaṇena vā ।।

surayā madhunā vātha yathā-sātmyam upācaret ।
bhojyāni kalpayed ūrdhvaṃ grāhi-dīpana-pācanaiḥ ।।

urayā madhunā cātha
bāla-bilva-śaṭhī-dhānya-hiṅgu-vṛkṣāmla-dāḍimaiḥ ।
palāśa-hapuṣājājī-yavānī-viḍa-saindhavaiḥ ।।

laghunā pañca-mūlena pañca-kolena pāṭhayā ।
śāliparṇī-balā-bilvaiḥ pṛśniparṇyā ca sādhitā ।।

dāḍimāmlā hitā peyā kapha-pitte samulbaṇe ।
abhayā-pippalī-mūla-bilvair vātānulomanī ।।

vibaddhaṃ doṣa-bahulo dīptāgnir yo atisāryate ।
kṛṣṇā-viḍaṅga-tri-phalā-kaṣāyais taṃ virecayet ।।

peyāṃ yuñjyād viriktasya vāta-ghnair dīpanaiḥ kṛtām ।
āme pariṇate yas tu dīpte agnāv upaveśyate ।।

sa-phena-picchaṃ sa-rujaṃ sa-vibandhaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।
alpālpam alpa-śamalaṃ nir-viḍ vā sa-pravāhikam ।।

lpālpam alpaṃ sa-malaṃ
dadhi-taila-ghṛta-kṣīraiḥ sa śuṇṭhīṃ sa-guḍāṃ pibet ।
svinnāni guḍa-tailena bhakṣayed badarāṇi vā ।।

gāḍha-viḍ-vihitaiḥ śākair bahu-snehais tathā rasaiḥ ।
kṣudhitaṃ bhojayed enaṃ dadhi-dāḍima-sādhitaiḥ ।।

adhi-dāḍima-saṃskṛtaiḥ
śāly-odanaṃ tilair māṣair mudgair vā sādhu sādhitam ।
śaṭhyā mūlaka-potāyāḥ pāṭhāyāḥ svastikasya vā ।।

śuṇṭhyā mūlaka-potāyāḥ
sūṣā-yavānī-karkāru-kṣīriṇī-cirbhaṭasya vā ।
upodakāyā jīvantyā vākucyā vāstukasya vā ।।

suvarcalāyāś cuñcor vā loṇikāyā rasair api ।
kūrma-vartaka-lopāka-śikhi-tittiri-kaukkuṭaiḥ ।।

-śikhi-tittiri-dakṣa-jaiḥ
bilva-mustākṣi-bhaiṣajya-dhātakī-puṣpa-nāgaraiḥ ।
pakvātīsāra-jit takre yavāgūr dādhikī tathā ।।

kapittha-kacchurā-phañjī-yūthikā-vaṭa-śelu-jaiḥ ।
dāḍimī-śaṇa-kārpāsī-śālmalīnāṃ ca pallavaiḥ ।।

-śālmalī-moca-pallavaiḥ
kalko bilva-śalāṭūnāṃ tila-kalkaś ca tat-samaḥ ।
dadhnaḥ saro amlaḥ sa-snehaḥ khalo hanti pravāhikām ।।

maricaṃ dhanikājājī tintiḍīkaṃ śaṭhī viḍam ।
dāḍimaṃ dhātakī pāṭhā tri-phalā pañca-kolakam ।।

yāva-śūkaṃ kapitthāmra-jambū-madhyaṃ sa-dīpyakam ।
piṣṭaiḥ ṣaḍ-guṇa-bilvais tair dadhni mudga-rase guḍe ।।

snehe ca yamake siddhaḥ khalo ayam a-parājitaḥ ।
dīpanaḥ pācano grāhī rucyo bimbiśi-nāśanaḥ ।।

kolānāṃ bāla-bilvānāṃ kalkaiḥ śāli-yavasya ca ।
mudga-māṣa-tilānāṃ ca dhānya-yūṣaṃ prakalpayet ।।

aikadhyaṃ yamake bhṛṣṭaṃ dadhi-dāḍima-sārikam ।
varcaḥ-kṣaye śuṣka-mukhaṃ śāly-annaṃ tena bhojayet ।।

dadhnaḥ saraṃ vā yamake bhṛṣṭaṃ sa-guḍa-nāgaram ।
surāṃ vā yamake bhṛṣṭāṃ vyañjanārthaṃ prayojayet ।।

phalāmlaṃ yamake bhṛṣṭaṃ yūṣaṃ gṛñjanakasya vā ।
bhṛṣṭān vā yamake saktūn khāded vyoṣāvacūrṇitān ।।

māṣān su-siddhāṃs tad-vad vā ghṛta-maṇḍopasevanān ।
rasaṃ su-siddha-pūtaṃ vā chāga-meṣāntar-ādhi-jam ।।

asaṃ su-siddhaṃ pūtaṃ vā
paced dāḍima-sārāmlaṃ sa-dhānya-sneha-nāgaram ।
rakta-śāly-odanaṃ tena bhuñjānaḥ prapibaṃś ca tam ।।

varcaḥ-kṣaya-kṛtair āśu vikāraiḥ parimucyate ।
bāla-bilvaṃ guḍaṃ tailaṃ pippalīṃ viśva-bheṣajam ।।

ippalī-viśva-bheṣajam
lihyād vāte pratihate sa-śūlaḥ sa-pravāhikaḥ ।
valkalaṃ śābaraṃ puṣpaṃ dhātakyā badarī-dalam ।।

a-śūle sa-pravāhike hātakyā badarī-phalam
eraṇḍa-bilva-yava-gokṣurakāmla-siddhāṃ pathyāṃ lihan madhu-yutām atha vā guḍena ।
kṛcchra-pravṛttam ati-śūlam asṛg-vimiśraṃ hanyād avaśyam atisāram udīrṇa-vegam ।।

।।

pibed dadhi-sara-kṣaudra-kapittha-sva-rasāplutam ।
vibaddha-vāta-varcās tu bahu-śūla-pravāhikaḥ ।।

sa-rakta-picchas tṛṣṇārtaḥ kṣīra-sauhityam arhati ।
yamakasyopari kṣīraṃ dhāroṣṇaṃ vā prayojayet ।।

śṛtam eraṇḍa-mūlena bāla-bilvena vā punaḥ ।
payasy utkvāthya mustānāṃ viṃśatiṃ tri-guṇe ambhasi ।।

iṃśatiṃ tri-guṇāmbhasi
kṣīrāvaśiṣṭaṃ tat pītaṃ hanyād āmaṃ sa-vedanam ।
pippalyāḥ pibataḥ sūkṣmaṃ rajo marica-janma vā ।।

cira-kālānuṣaktāpi naśyaty āśu pravāhikā ।
nir-āma-rūpaṃ śūlārtaṃ laṅghanādyaiś ca karṣitam ।।

rūkṣa-koṣṭham apekṣyāgniṃ sa-kṣāraṃ pāyayed ghṛtam ।
siddhaṃ dadhi-surā-maṇḍe daśa-mūlasya cāmbhasi ।।

aśa-mūlasya vāmbhasi
sindhūttha-pañca-kolābhyāṃ tailaṃ sadyo arti-nāśanam ।
ṣaḍbhiḥ śuṇṭhyāḥ palair dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ granthy-agni-saindhavāt ।।

taila-prasthaṃ paced dadhnā niḥ-sāraka-rujāpaham ।
ekato māṃsa-dugdhājyaṃ purīṣa-graha-śūla-jit ।।

pānānuvāsanābhyaṅga-prayuktaṃ tailam ekataḥ ।
tad dhi vāta-jitām agryaṃ śūlaṃ ca vi-guṇo anilaḥ ।।

dhātv-antaropamardeddhaś calo vyāpī sva-dhāma-gaḥ ।
tailaṃ mandānalasyāpi yuktyā śarma-karaṃ param ।।

hātv-antaropamardād vai hātv-antaropamardena vāyv-āśaye sa-taile hi bimbiśir nāvatiṣṭhate ।।

kṣīṇe male svāyatana-cyuteṣu doṣāntareṣv īraṇa eka-vīre ।
ko niṣṭanan prāṇiti koṣṭha-śūlī nāntar-bahis-taila-paro yadi syāt ।।
guda-rug-bhraṃśayor yuñjyāt sa-kṣīraṃ sādhitaṃ haviḥ ।।
rase kolāmla-cāṅgeryor dadhni piṣṭe ca nāgare ।
tair eva cāmlaiḥ saṃyojya siddhaṃ su-ślakṣṇa-kalkitaiḥ ।।

air eva cāmlaiḥ saṃyuktaiḥ
dhānyoṣaṇa-viḍājājī-pañca-kolaka-dāḍimaiḥ ।
yojayet sneha-vastiṃ vā daśa-mūlena sādhitam ।।

śaṭhī-śatāhvā-kuṣṭhair vā vacayā citrakeṇa vā ।
pravāhaṇe guda-bhraṃśe mūtrāghāte kaṭī-grahe ।।

madhurāmlaiḥ śṛtaṃ tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vāpy anuvāsanam ।
praveśayed gudaṃ dhvastam abhyaktaṃ sveditaṃ mṛdu ।।

kuryāc ca go-phaṇā-bandhaṃ madhya-cchidreṇa carmaṇā ।
pañca-mūlasya mahataḥ kvāthaṃ kṣīre vipācayet ।।

vāthaṃ kṣīreṇa pācayet
unduruṃ cāntra-rahitaṃ tena vāta-ghna-kalka-vat ।
tailaṃ paced guda-bhraṃśaṃ pānābhyaṅgena taj jayet ।।

paitte tu sāme tīkṣṇoṣṇa-varjyaṃ prāg iva laṅghanam ।
tṛḍ-vān pibet ṣaḍ-aṅgāmbu sa-bhūnimbaṃ sa-śārivam ।।

peyādi kṣudhitasyānnam agni-saṃdhukṣaṇaṃ hitam ।
bṛhaty-ādi-gaṇābhīru-dvi-balā-śūrpaparṇibhiḥ ।।

pāyayed anubandhe tu sa-kṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbhasā ।
kuṭajasya phalaṃ piṣṭaṃ sa-valkaṃ sa-ghuṇapriyam ।।

a-kṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbunā atsakasya phalaṃ piṣṭaṃ
pāṭhā-vatsaka-bīja-tvag-dārvī-granthika-śuṇṭhi vā ।
kvāthaṃ vātiviṣā-bilva-vatsakodīcya-musta-jam ।।

atha-vātiviṣā-mūrvā-niśendrayava-tārkṣya-jam ।
sa-madhv-ativiṣā-śuṇṭhī-mustendrayava-kaṭphalam ।।

palaṃ vatsaka-bījasya śrapayitvā rasaṃ pibet ।
yo rasāśī jayec chīghraṃ sa paittaṃ jaṭharāmayam ।।

mustā-kaṣāyam evaṃ vā piben madhu-samāyutam ।
sa-kṣaudraṃ śālmalī-vṛnta-kaṣāyaṃ vā himāhvayam ।।

kirātatiktakaṃ mustaṃ vatsakaṃ sa-rasāñjanam ।
kaṭaṅkaṭerī hrīveraṃ bilva-madhyaṃ durālabhā ।।

tilā moca-rasaṃ lodhraṃ samaṅgā kamalotpalam ।
nāgaraṃ dhātakī-puṣpaṃ dāḍimasya tvag utpalam ।।

ardha-ślokaiḥ smṛtā yogāḥ sa-kṣaudrās taṇḍulāmbunā ।
niśendrayava-lodhrailā-kvāthaḥ pakvātisāra-jit ।।

-kvāthaḥ pakvātisāra-nut
nāgarātiviṣā-mustā-bhūnimbāmṛta-vatsakaiḥ ।
sarva-jvara-haraḥ kvāthaḥ sarvātīsāra-nāśanaḥ ।।

guḍūcy-ativiṣā-dhānya-śuṇṭhī-bilvābda-vālakaiḥ ।
pāṭhā-bhūnimba-kuṭaja-candanośīra-padmakaiḥ ।।

kaṣāyaḥ śitalaḥ peyo jvarātīsāra-śāntaye ।
hṛl-lāsā-rocaka-cchardi-pipāsā-dāha-nāśanaḥ ।।

lodhrāmbaṣṭhā-priyaṅgv-ādi-gaṇāṃs tad-vat pṛthak pibet ।
kaṭvaṅga-valka-yaṣṭy-āhva-phalinī-dāḍimāṅkuraiḥ ।।

peyā-vilepī-khalakān kuryāt sa-dadhi-dāḍimān ।
tad-vad dadhittha-bilvāmra-jambū-madhyaiḥ prakalpayet ।।

ajā-payaḥ prayoktavyaṃ nir-āme tena cec chamaḥ ।
doṣādhikyān na jāyeta balinaṃ taṃ virecayet ।।

vyatyāsena śakṛd-raktam upaveśyeta yo api vā ।
palāśa-phala-niryūhaṃ yuktaṃ vā payasā pibet ।।

tato anu koṣṇaṃ pātavyaṃ kṣīram eva yathā-balam ।
pravāhite tena male praśāmyaty udarāmayaḥ ।।

palāśa-vat prayojyā vā trāyamāṇā viśodhanī ।
saṃsargyāṃ kriyamāṇāyāṃ śūlaṃ yady anuvartate ।।

rāyamāṇā viśodhane
sruta-doṣasya taṃ śīghraṃ yathā-vahny anuvāsayet ।
śatapuṣpā-varībhyāṃ ca bilvena madhukena ca ।।

taila-pādaṃ payo-yuktaṃ pakvam anvāsanaṃ ghṛtam ।
a-śāntāv ity atīsāre picchā-vastiḥ paraṃ hitaḥ ।।

pariveṣṭya kuśair ārdrair ārdra-vṛntāni śālmaleḥ ।
kṛṣṇa-mṛttikayālipya svedayed go-mayāgninā ।।

mṛc-choṣe tāni saṃkṣudya tat-piṇḍaṃ muṣṭi-saṃmitam ।
mardayet payasaḥ prasthe pūtenāsthāpayet tataḥ ।।

nata-yaṣṭy-āhva-kalkājya-kṣaudra-taila-vatānu ca ।
snāto bhuñjīta payasā jāṅgalena rasena vā ।।

pittātisāra-jvara-śopha-gulma-samīraṇāsra-grahaṇī-vikārān ।
jayaty ayaṃ śīghram ati-pravṛttiṃ virecanāsthāpanayoś ca vastiḥ ।।

kaṭvaṅga-bilva-jaṃ tv asthi kapitthaṃ surasāñjanam ।
lākṣā-haridre hrīveraṃ kaṭphalaṃ śukanāsikā ।।

lodhraṃ moca-rasaṃ mustaṃ dhātakī vaṭa-śuṅgakān ।
piṣṭvā taṇḍula-toyena vaṭakān akṣa-saṃmitān ।।

pibet tenaiva toyena jvarātīsāra-nāśanaḥ ।
rakta-prasādano hy eṣa śophātīsāra-nāśanaḥ ।।

phāṇitaṃ kuṭajotthaṃ ca sarvātīsāra-nāśanam ।
vatsakādi-samāyuktaṃ sāmbaṣṭhādi sa-mākṣikam ।।

nī-ruṅ-nir-āmaṃ dīptāgner api sāsraṃ cirotthitam ।
nānā-varṇam atīsāraṃ puṭa-pākair upācaret ।।

tvak-piṇḍād dīrghavṛntasya śrīparṇī-pattra-saṃvṛtāt ।
mṛl-liptād agninā svinnād rasaṃ niṣpīḍitaṃ himam ।।

atīsārī pibed yuktaṃ madhunā sitayātha-vā ।
evaṃ kṣīri-druma-tvagbhis tat-prarohaiś ca kalpayet ।।

vaṃ kṣīra-druma-tvagbhis
kaṭvaṅga-tvag-ghṛta-yutā sveditā saliloṣmaṇā ।
sa-kṣaudrā hanty atīsāraṃ bala-vantam api drutam ।।

pittātīsārī seveta pittalāny eva yaḥ punaḥ ।
raktātīsāraṃ kurute tasya pittaṃ sa-tṛḍ-jvaram ।।

dāruṇaṃ guda-pākaṃ ca tatra cchāgaṃ payo hitam ।
padmotpala-samaṅgābhiḥ śṛtaṃ moca-rasena ca ।।

śārivā-yaṣṭi-lodhrair vā prasavair vā vaṭādi-jaiḥ ।
sa-kṣaudra-śarkaraṃ pāne bhojane guda-secane ।।

tad-vad rasādayo an-amlāḥ sājyāḥ pānānnayor hitāḥ ।
kāśmarya-phala-yūṣaś ca kiñ-cid-amlaḥ sa-śarkaraḥ ।।

payasy ardhodake chāge hrīverotpala-nāgaraiḥ ।
peyā raktātisāra-ghnī pṛśniparṇī-rasānvitā ।।

prāg-bhaktaṃ nava-nītaṃ vā lihyān madhu-sitā-yutam ।
baliny asre asram evājaṃ mārgaṃ vā ghṛta-bharjitam ।।

kṣīrānu-pānaṃ kṣīrāśī try-ahaṃ kṣīrodbhavaṃ ghṛtam ।
kapiñjala-rasāśī vā lihann ārogyam aśnute ।।

pītvā śatāvarī-kalkaṃ kṣīreṇa kṣīra-bhojanaḥ ।
raktātīsāraṃ hanty āśu tayā vā sādhitaṃ ghṛtam ।।

lākṣā-nāgara-vaidehī-kaṭukā-dārvi-valkalaiḥ ।
sarpiḥ sendrayavaiḥ siddhaṃ peyā-maṇḍāvacāritam ।।

atīsāraṃ jayec chīghraṃ tri-doṣam api dāruṇam ।
kṛṣṇa-mṛc-chaṅkha-yaṣṭy-āhva-kṣaudrāsṛk-taṇḍulodakam ।।

jayaty asraṃ priyaṅguś ca taṇḍulāmbu-madhu-plutā ।
kalkas tilānāṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ śarkarā-pāñcabhāgikaḥ ।।

śarkarā-bhāga-saṃyutaḥ
ājena payasā pītaḥ sadyo raktaṃ niyacchati ।
pītvā sa-śarkarā-kṣaudraṃ candanaṃ taṇḍulāmbunā ।।

dāha-tṛṣṇā-pramohebhyo rakta-srāvāc ca mucyate ।
gudasya dāhe pāke vā seka-lepā hitā himāḥ ।।

āha-tṛṣṇā-pramehebhyo ekā lepā hitā himāḥ
alpālpaṃ bahu-śo raktaṃ sa-śūlam upaveśyate ।
yadā vibaddho vāyuś ca kṛcchrāc carati vā na vā ।।

picchā-vastiṃ tadā tasya pūrvoktam upakalpayet ।
pallavān jarjarī-kṛtya śiṃśipā-kovidārayoḥ ।।

paced yavāṃś ca sa kvāthe ghṛta-kṣīra-samanvitaḥ ।
picchā-srutau guda-bhraṃśe pravāhaṇa-rujāsu vā ।।

picchā-vastiḥ prayoktavyaḥ kṣata-kṣīṇa-balāvahaḥ ।
prapauṇḍarīka-siddhena sarpiṣā cānuvāsanam ।।

raktaṃ viṭ-sahitaṃ pūrvaṃ paścād vā yo atisāryate ।
śatāvarī-ghṛtaṃ tasya lehārtham upakalpayet ।।

śarkarārdhāṃśakaṃ līḍhaṃ nava-nītaṃ navoddhṛtam ।
kṣaudra-pādaṃ jayec chīghraṃ taṃ vikāraṃ hitāśinaḥ ।।

nyagrodhodumbarāśvattha-śuṅgān āpothya vāsayet ।
aho-rātraṃ jale tapte ghṛtaṃ tenāmbhasā pacet ।।

tad ardha-śarkarā-yuktaṃ lehayet kṣaudra-pādikam ।
adho vā yadi vāpy urdhvaṃ yasya raktaṃ pravartate ।।

dho vā yadi vāty-urdhvaṃ
śleṣmātīsāre vātoktaṃ viśeṣād āma-pācanam ।
kartavyam anubandhe asya pibet paktvāgni-dīpanam ।।

bilva-karkaṭikā-musta-prāṇadā-viśva-bheṣajam ।
vacā-viḍaṅga-bhūtīka-dhānakāmaradāru vā ।।

-dhānyakāmaradāru vā
atha-vā pippalī-mūla-pippalī-dvaya-citrakam ।
pāṭhāgni-vatsaka-granthi-tiktā-śuṇṭhī-vacābhayāḥ ।।

-pippalī-dvaya-citrakān
kvathitā yadi vā piṣṭāḥ śleṣmātīsāra-bheṣajam ।
sauvarcala-vacā-vyoṣa-hiṅgu-prativiṣābhayāḥ ।।

pibec chleṣmātisārārtaś cūrṇitāḥ koṣṇa-vāriṇā ।
madhyaṃ līḍhvā kapitthasya sa-vyoṣa-kṣaudra-śarkaram ।।

a-kṣaudraṃ vyoṣa-śarkaram
kaṭphalaṃ madhu-yuktaṃ vā mucyate jaṭharāmayāt ।
kaṇāṃ madhu-yutāṃ līḍhvā takraṃ pītvā sa-citrakam ।।

bhuktvā vā bāla-bilvāni vyapohaty udarāmayam ।
pāṭhā-moca-rasāmbhoda-dhātakī-bilva-nāgaram ।।

su-kṛcchram apy atīsāraṃ guḍa-takreṇa nāśayet ।
yavānī-pippalī-mūla-cāturjātaka-nāgaraiḥ ।।

maricāgni-jalājājī-dhānya-sauvarcalaiḥ samaiḥ ।
vṛṣāmla-dhātakī-kṛṣṇā-bilva-dāḍima-dīpyakaiḥ ।।

c vṛkṣāmla-dhātakī-kṛṣṇā- c -bilva-dāḍima-tindukaiḥ
tri-guṇaiḥ ṣaḍ-guṇa-sitaiḥ kapitthāṣṭa-guṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ ।
cūrṇo atīsāra-grahaṇī-kṣaya-gulma-galāmayān ।।

ri-guṇaiḥ ṣaḍ-guṇa-site apitthe aṣṭa-guṇe kṛtaḥ 
-kṣaya-gulmodarāmayān
kāsa-śvāsāgni-sādārśaḥ-pīnasā-rocakāñ jayet ।
karṣonmitā tavakṣīrī cāturjātaṃ dvi-kārṣikam ।।

arṣonmitaṃ tavakṣīrī- -cāturjātaṃ dvi-kārṣikam
yavānī-dhānyakājājī-granthi-vyoṣaṃ palāṃśakam ।
palāni dāḍimād aṣṭau sitāyāś caikataḥ kṛtaḥ ।।

avānī-dhānyakājāji ranthi-vyoṣaṃ palāṃśakam
guṇaiḥ kapitthāṣṭaka-vac cūrṇo ayaṃ dāḍimāṣṭakaḥ ।
bhojyo vātātisāroktair yathāvasthaṃ khalādibhiḥ ।।

sa-viḍaṅgaḥ sa-maricaḥ sa-kapitthaḥ sa-nāgaraḥ ।
cāṅgerī-takra-kolāmlaḥ khalaḥ śleṣmātisāra-jit ।।

kṣīṇe śleṣmaṇi pūrvoktam amlaṃ lākṣādi ṣaṭ-palam ।
purāṇaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ dadyād yavāgū-maṇḍa-miśritam ।।

kaṭphalaṃ madhukaṃ lodhraṃ tvag-dāḍima-phalasya ca ।
vāta-pittātisāra-ghnaṃ pibet taṇḍula-vāriṇā ।।

mustaṃ sātiviṣā dārvī vacā śuṇṭhī ca tat-samam ।
kaṣāyaṃ kṣaudra-saṃyuktaṃ śleṣma-vātātisāriṇe ।।

pītadāru vacā lodhraṃ kaliṅga-phala-nāgaram ।
dāḍimāmbu-yutaṃ dadyāt pitta-śleṣmātisāriṇe ।।

vāta-śleṣma-vibandhe vā sravaty ati kaphe api vā ।
śūle pravāhikāyāṃ vā picchā-vastiḥ praśasyate ।।

āta-śleṣma-vibandhe ca
vacā-bilva-kaṇā-kuṣṭha-śatāhvā-lavaṇānvitaḥ ।
bilva-tailena tailena vacādyaiḥ sādhitena vā ।।

bahu-śaḥ kapha-vātārte koṣṇenānvāsanaṃ hitam ।
kṣīṇe kaphe gude dīrgha-kālātīsāra-dur-bale ।।

anilaḥ prabalo avaśyaṃ sva-sthāna-sthaḥ prajāyate ।
sa balī sahasā hanyāt tasmāt taṃ tvarayā jayet ।।

vāyor an-antaraṃ pittaṃ pittasyān-antaraṃ kapham ।
jayet pūrvaṃ trayāṇāṃ vā bhaved yo bala-vat-tamaḥ ।।

bhī-śokābhyām api calaḥ śīghraṃ kupyaty atas tayoḥ ।
kāryā kriyā vāta-harā harṣaṇāśvāsanāni ca ।।

yasyoccārād vinā mūtraṃ pavano vā pravartate ।
dīptāgner laghu-koṣṭhasya śāntas tasyodarāmayaḥ ।।

cikitsāsthāna
grahaṇīm āśritaṃ doṣam a-jīrṇa-vad upācaret ।
atīsārokta-vidhinā tasyāmaṃ ca vipācayet ।।

anna-kāle yavāgv-ādi pañca-kolādibhir yutam ।
vitaret paṭu-laghv-annaṃ punar yogāṃś ca dīpanān ।।

dadyāt sātiviṣāṃ peyām āme sāmlāṃ sa-nāgarām ।
pāne atīsāra-vihitaṃ vāri takraṃ surādi ca ।।

grahaṇī-doṣiṇāṃ takraṃ dīpana-grāhi-lāghavāt ।
pathyaṃ madhura-pāki-tvān na ca pitta-pradūṣaṇam ।।

kaṣāyoṣṇa-vikāśi-tvād rūkṣa-tvāc ca kaphe hitam ।
vāte svādv-amla-sāndra-tvāt sadyaskam a-vidāhi tat ।।

aṣāyoṣṇa-vikāṣi-tvād
caturṇāṃ prastham amlānāṃ try-ūṣaṇāc ca pala-trayam ।
lavaṇānāṃ ca catvāri śarkarāyāḥ palāṣṭakam ।।

tac cūrṇaṃ śāka-sūpānna-rāgādiṣv avacārayet ।
kāsā-jīrṇā-ruci-śvāsa-hṛt-pāṇḍu-plīha-gulma-nut ।।

-hṛt-pārśvāmaya-śūla-nut -hṛt-pāṇḍv-āmaya-śūla-nut
nāgarātiviṣā-mustaṃ pākyam āma-haraṃ pibet ।
uṣṇāmbunā vā tat-kalkaṃ nāgaraṃ vātha-vābhayām ।।

sa-saindhavaṃ vacādiṃ vā tad-van madirayātha-vā ।
varcasy āme sa-pravāhe pibed vā dāḍimāmbunā ।।

viḍena lavaṇaṃ piṣṭaṃ bilva-citraka-nāgaram ।
sāme kaphānile koṣṭha-ruk-kare koṣṇa-vāriṇā ।।

kaliṅga-hiṅgv-ativiṣā-vacā-sauvarcalābhayam ।
chardi-hṛd-roga-śūleṣu peyam uṣṇena vāriṇā ।।

pathyā-sauvarcalājājī-cūrṇaṃ marica-saṃyutam ।
pippalīṃ nāgaraṃ pāṭhāṃ śārivāṃ bṛhatī-dvayam ।।

citrakaṃ kauṭajaṃ kṣāraṃ tathā lavaṇa-pañcakam ।
cūrṇī-kṛtaṃ dadhi-surā-tan-maṇḍoṣṇāmbu-kāñjikaiḥ ।।

pibed agni-vivṛddhy-arthaṃ koṣṭha-vāta-haraṃ param ।
paṭūni pañca dvau kṣārau maricaṃ pañca-kolakam ।।

dīpyakaṃ hiṅgu guṭikā bījapūra-rase kṛtā ।
kola-dāḍima-toye vā paraṃ pācana-dīpanī ।।

tālīśa-pattra-cavikā-maricānāṃ palaṃ palam ।
kṛṣṇā-tan-mūlayor dve dve pale śuṇṭhī-pala-trayam ।।

catur-jātam uśīraṃ ca karṣāṃśaṃ ślakṣṇa-cūrṇitam ।
guḍena vaṭakān kṛtvā tri-guṇena sadā bhajet ।।

madya-yūṣa-rasāriṣṭa-mastu-peyā-payo-'nupaḥ ।
vāta-śleṣmātmanāṃ chardi-grahaṇī-pārśva-hṛd-rujām ।।

jvara-śvayathu-pāṇḍu-tva-gulma-pānātyayārśasām ।
praseka-pīnasa-śvāsa-kāsānāṃ ca nivṛttaye ।।

abhayāṃ nāgara-sthāne dadyāt tatraiva viḍ-grahe ।
chardy-ādiṣu ca paitteṣu catur-guṇa-sitānvitāḥ ।।

adyād atraiva viḍ-grahe
pakvena vaṭakāḥ kāryā guḍena sitayāpi vā ।
paraṃ hi vahni-saṃparkāl laghimānaṃ bhajanti te ।।

athainaṃ paripakvāmaṃ māruta-grahaṇī-gadam ।
dīpanīya-yutaṃ sarpiḥ pāyayed alpa-śo bhiṣak ।।

thainaṃ paripakvāma- -māruta-grahaṇī-gadam
kiñ-cit-saṃdhukṣite tv agnau sakta-viṇ-mūtra-mārutam ।
dvy-ahaṃ try-ahaṃ vā saṃsnehya svinnābhyaktaṃ nirūhayet ।।

tata eraṇḍa-tailena sarpiṣā tailvakena vā ।
sa-kṣāreṇānile śānte srasta-doṣaṃ virecayet ।।

śuddha-rūkṣāśayaṃ baddha-varcaskaṃ cānuvāsayet ।
dīpanīyāmla-vāta-ghna-siddha-tailena taṃ tataḥ ।।

nirūḍhaṃ ca viriktaṃ ca samyak cāpy anuvāsitam ।
laghv-anna-pratisaṃyuktaṃ sarpir abhyāsayet punaḥ ।।

amyag vāpy anuvāsitam
pañca-mūlābhayā-vyoṣa-pippalī-mūla-saindhavaiḥ ।
rāsnā-kṣāra-dvayājājī-viḍaṅga-śaṭhibhir ghṛtam ।।

śuktena mātuluṅgasya sva-rasenārdrakasya ca ।
śuṣka-mūlaka-kolāmla-cukrikā-dāḍimasya ca ।।

takra-mastu-surā-maṇḍa-sauvīraka-tuṣodakaiḥ ।
kāñjikena ca tat pakvam agni-dīpti-karaṃ param ।।

śūla-gulmodara-śvāsa-kāsānila-kaphāpaham ।
sa-bījapūraka-rasaṃ siddhaṃ vā pāyayed ghṛtam ।।

tailam abhyañjanārthaṃ ca siddham ebhiś calāpaham ।
eteṣām auṣadhānāṃ vā pibec cūrṇaṃ sukhāmbunā ।।

vāte śleṣmāvṛte sāme kaphe vā vāyunoddhate ।
agner nirvāpakaṃ pittaṃ rekeṇa vamanena vā ।।

hatvā tikta-laghu-grāhi-dīpanair a-vidāhibhiḥ ।
annaiḥ saṃdhukṣayed agniṃ cūrṇaiḥ snehaiś ca tiktakaiḥ ।।

paṭola-nimba-trāyantī-tiktā-tiktaka-parpaṭam ।
kuṭaja-tvak-phalaṃ mūrvā madhu-śigru-phalaṃ vacā ।।

dārvī-tvak-padmakośīra-yavānī-musta-candanam ।
saurāṣṭry-ativiṣā-vyoṣa-tvag-elā-pattra-dāru ca ।।

cūrṇitaṃ madhunā lehyaṃ peyaṃ madyair jalena vā ।
hṛt-pāṇḍu-grahaṇī-roga-gulma-śūlā-ruci-jvarān ।।

kāmalāṃ saṃnipātaṃ ca mukha-rogāṃś ca nāśayet ।
bhūnimba-kaṭukā-mustā-try-ūṣaṇendrayavān samān ।।

dvau citrakād vatsaka-tvag-bhāgān ṣo-ḍaśa cūrṇayet ।
guḍa-śītāmbunā pītaṃ grahaṇī-doṣa-gulma-nut ।।

kāmalā-jvara-pāṇḍu-tva-mehā-rucy-atisāra-jit ।
nāgarātiviṣā-mustā-pāṭhā-bilvaṃ rasāñjanam ।।

-mehā-rucy-atisāra-nut
kuṭaja-tvak-phalaṃ tiktā dhātakī ca kṛtaṃ rajaḥ ।
kṣaudra-taṇḍula-vāribhyāṃ paittike grahaṇī-gade ।।

pravāhikārśo-guda-rug-raktotthāneṣu ceṣyate ।
candanaṃ padmakośīraṃ pāṭhāṃ mūrvāṃ kuṭannaṭam ।।

ṣaḍgranthā-śārivāsphotā-saptaparṇāṭarūṣakān ।
paṭolodumbarāśvattha-vaṭa-plakṣa-kapītanān ।।

-vaṭa-plakṣa-kapītanam
kaṭukāṃ rohiṇīṃ mustāṃ nimbaṃ ca dvi-palāṃśakān ।
droṇe apāṃ sādhayet tena pacet sarpiḥ picūnmitaiḥ ।।

kirātatiktendrayava-vīrā-māgadhikotpalaiḥ ।
pitta-grahaṇyāṃ tat peyaṃ kuṣṭhoktaṃ tiktakaṃ ca yat ।।

grahaṇyāṃ śleṣma-duṣṭāyāṃ tīkṣṇaiḥ pracchardane kṛte ।
kaṭv-amla-lavaṇa-kṣāraiḥ kramād agniṃ vivardhayet ।।

pañca-kolābhayā-dhānya-pāṭhā-gandha-palāśakaiḥ ।
bījapūra-pragāḍhaiś ca siddhaiḥ peyādi kalpayet ।।

droṇaṃ madhūka-puṣpāṇāṃ viḍaṅgaṃ ca tato ardhataḥ ।
citrakasya tato ardhaṃ ca tathā bhallātakāḍhakam ।।

mañjiṣṭhāṣṭa-palaṃ caitaj jala-droṇa-traye pacet ।
droṇa-śeṣaṃ śṛtaṃ śītaṃ madhv-ardhāḍhaka-saṃyutam ।।

elā-mṛṇālāgurubhiś candanena ca rūṣite ।
kumbhe māsaṃ sthitaṃ jātam āsavaṃ taṃ prayojayet ।।

umbhe māsa-sthitaṃ jātam
grahaṇīṃ dīpayaty eṣa bṛṃhaṇaḥ pitta-rakta-nut ।
śoṣa-kuṣṭha-kilāsānāṃ pramehāṇāṃ ca nāśanaḥ ।।

ṛṃhaṇo rakta-pitta-nut
madhūka-puṣpa-sva-rasaṃ śṛtam ardha-kṣayī-kṛtam ।
kṣaudra-pāda-yutaṃ śītaṃ pūrva-vat saṃnidhāpayet ।।

adhūka-puṣpa-kuḍavaṃ
tat piban grahaṇī-doṣān jayet sarvān hitāśanaḥ ।
tad-vad drākṣekṣu-kharjūra-sva-rasān āsutān pibet ।।

hiṅgu-tiktā-vacā-mādrī-pāṭhendrayava-gokṣuram ।
pañca-kolaṃ ca karṣāṃśaṃ palāṃśaṃ paṭu-pañcakam ।।

ghṛta-taila-dvi-kuḍave dadhnaḥ prastha-dvaye ca tat ।
āpothya kvāthayed agnau mṛdāv anugate rase ।।

antar-dhūmaṃ tato dagdhvā cūrṇī-kṛtya ghṛtāplutam ।
pibet pāṇi-talaṃ tasmiñ jīrṇe syān madhurāśanaḥ ।।

vāta-śleṣmāmayān sarvān hanyād viṣa-garāṃś ca saḥ ।
bhūnimbaṃ rohiṇīṃ tiktāṃ paṭolaṃ nimba-parpaṭam ।।

dagdhvā māhiṣa-mūtreṇa pibed agni-vivardhanam ।
dve haridre vacā kuṣṭhaṃ citrakaḥ kaṭu-rohiṇī ।।

mustā ca cchāga-mūtreṇa siddhaḥ kṣāro agni-vardhanaḥ ।
catuḥ-palaṃ sudhā-kāṇḍāt tri-palaṃ lavaṇa-trayāt ।।

ri-phalā-lavaṇāni ca
vārtāka-kuḍavaṃ cārkād aṣṭau dve citrakāt pale ।
dagdhvā rasena vārtākād guṭikā bhojanottarāḥ ।।

ārtākāt kuḍavaṃ cārkād
bhuktam annaṃ pacanty āśu kāsa-śvāsārśasāṃ hitāḥ ।
viṣūcikā-pratiśyāya-hṛd-roga-śamanāś ca tāḥ ।।

mātuluṅga-śaṭhī-rāsnā-kaṭu-traya-harītaki ।
svarjikā-yāva-śūkākhyau kṣārau pañca-paṭūni ca ।।

-kaṭu-traya-harītakīḥ
sukhāmbu-pītaṃ tac-cūrṇaṃ bala-varṇāgni-vardhanam ।
ślaiṣmike grahaṇī-doṣe sa-vāte tair ghṛtaṃ pacet ।।

dhānvantaraṃ ṣaṭ-palaṃ ca bhallātaka-ghṛtābhayam ।
viḍa-kācoṣa-lavaṇa-svarjikā-yāva-śūka-jān ।।

saptalāṃ kaṇṭakārīṃ ca citrakaṃ caikato dahet ।
sapta-kṛtvaḥ srutasyāsya kṣārasyārdhāḍhake pacet ।।

āḍhakaṃ sarpiṣaḥ peyaṃ tad agni-bala-vṛddhaye ।
nicaye pañca karmāṇi yuñjyāc caitad yathā-balam ।।

praseke ślaiṣmike alpāgner dīpanaṃ rūkṣa-tiktakam ।
yojyaṃ kṛśasya vyatyāsāt snigdha-rūkṣaṃ kaphodaye ।।

kṣīṇa-kṣāma-śarīrasya dīpanaṃ sneha-saṃyutam ।
dīpanaṃ bahu-pittasya tiktaṃ madhurakair yutam ।।

sneho amla-lavaṇair yukto bahu-vātasya śasyate ।
sneham eva paraṃ vidyād dur-balānala-dīpanam ।।

nālaṃ sneha-samiddhasya śamāyānnaṃ su-gurv api ।
yo alpāgni-tvāt kaphe kṣīṇe varcaḥ pakvam api ślatham ।।

muñcet paṭv-auṣadha-yutaṃ sa pibed alpa-śo ghṛtam ।
tena sva-mārgam ānītaḥ sva-karmaṇi niyojitaḥ ।।

samāno dīpayaty agnim agneḥ saṃdhukṣako hi saḥ ।
purīṣaṃ yaś ca kṛcchreṇa kaṭhina-tvād vimuñcati ।।

gneḥ saṃdhukṣako hy asau
sa ghṛtaṃ lavaṇair yuktaṃ naro annāvagrahaṃ pibet ।
raukṣyān mande anale sarpis tailaṃ vā dīpanaiḥ pibet ।।

kṣāra-cūrṇāsavāriṣṭan mande snehāti-pānataḥ ।
udāvartāt tu yoktavyā nirūha-sneha-vastayaḥ ।।

dāvartāt prayoktavyā
doṣāti-vṛddhyā mande agnau saṃśuddho anna-vidhiṃ caret ।
vyādhi-muktasya mande agnau sarpir eva tu dīpanam ।।

aṃśuddho anna-vidhiṃ bhajet
adhvopavāsa-kṣāma-tvair yavāgvā pāyayed ghṛtam ।
annāvapīḍitaṃ balyaṃ dīpanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ ca tat ।।

dīrgha-kāla-prasaṅgāt tu kṣāma-kṣīṇa-kṛśān narān ।
prasahānāṃ rasaiḥ sāmlair bhojayet piśitāśinām ।।

laghūṣṇa-kaṭu-śodhi-tvād dīpayanty āśu te analam ।
māṃsopacita-māṃsa-tvāt paraṃ ca bala-vardhanāḥ ।।

aghūṣṇa-kaṭu-śodhi-tvair
snehāsava-surāriṣṭa-cūrṇa-kvātha-hitāśanaiḥ ।
samyak-prayuktair dehasya balam agneś ca vardhate ।।

dīpto yathaiva sthāṇuś ca bāhyo agniḥ sāra-dārubhiḥ ।
sa-snehair jāyate tad-vad āhāraiḥ koṣṭha-go analaḥ ।।

nā-bhojanena kāyāgnir dīpyate nāti-bhojanāt ।
yathā nir-indhano vahnir alpo vātīndhanāvṛtaḥ ।।

lpo vātīndhanānvitaḥ
yadā kṣīṇe kaphe pittaṃ sva-sthāne pavanānugam ।
pravṛddhaṃ vardhayaty agniṃ tadāsau sānilo analaḥ ।।

paktvānnam āśu dhātūṃś ca sarvān ojaś ca saṃkṣipan ।
mārayet syāt sa nā svastho bhukte jīrṇe tu tāmyati ।।

ārayet taṃ sa nā svastho
tṛṭ-kāsa-dāha-mūrchādyā vyādhayo aty-agni-saṃbhavāḥ ।
tam aty-agniṃ guru-snigdha-manda-sāndra-hima-sthiraiḥ ।।

anna-pānair nayec chāntiṃ dīptam agnim ivāmbubhiḥ ।
muhur muhur a-jīrṇe api bhojyāny asyopahārayet ।।

hojyāny asyopakalpayet
nir-indhano antaraṃ labdhvā yathainaṃ na vipādayet ।
kṛśarāṃ pāyasaṃ snigdhaṃ paiṣṭikaṃ guḍa-vaikṛtam ।।

athainaṃ na vipādayet
aśnīyād audakānūpa-piśitāni bhṛtāni ca ।
matsyān viśeṣataḥ ślakṣṇān sthira-toya-carāś ca ye ।।

āvikaṃ su-bhṛtaṃ māṃsam adyād aty-agni-vāraṇam ।
payaḥ saha-madhūcchiṣṭaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā tṛṣitaḥ pibet ।।

godhūma-cūrṇaṃ payasā bahu-sarpiḥ-pariplutam ।
ānūpa-rasa-yuktān vā snehāṃs taila-vivarjitān ।।

śyāmā-trivṛd-vipakvaṃ vā payo dadyād virecanam ।
a-sakṛt pitta-haraṇaṃ pāyasa-pratibhojanam ।।

yat kiñ-cid guru medyaṃ ca śleṣma-kāri ca bhojanam ।
sarvaṃ tad aty-agni-hitaṃ bhuktvā ca svapanaṃ divā ।।

āhāram agniḥ pacati doṣān āhāra-varjitaḥ ।
dhātūn kṣīṇeṣu doṣeṣu jīvitaṃ dhātu-saṃkṣaye ।।

etat prakṛtyaiva viruddham annaṃ saṃyoga-saṃskāra-vaśena cedam ।
ity-ādi a-vijñāya yatheṣṭa-ceṣṭāś caranti yat sāgni-balasya śaktiḥ ।।

tasmād agniṃ pālayet sarva-yatnais tasmin naṣṭe yāti nā nāśam eva ।
doṣair graste grasyate roga-saṃghair yukte tu syān nī-rujo dīrgha-jīvī ।।

cikitsāsthāna
liṅgāgra-suṣire samyag yonyāṃ vā saṃpraveśayet ।
mūtra-duḥkha-haraṃ mukhyaṃ karpūraṃ parisaṃkṣipet ।।

kṛcchre vāta-ghna-tailāktam adho nābheḥ samīra-je ।
su-snigdhaiḥ svedayed aṅgaṃ piṇḍa-sekāvagāhanaiḥ ।।

daśa-mūla-balairaṇḍa-yavābhīru-punarnavaiḥ ।
kulattha-kola-pattūra-vṛścīvopalabhedakaiḥ ।।

taila-sarpir-varāharkṣa-vasāḥ kvathita-kalkitaiḥ ।
sa-pañca-lavaṇāḥ siddhāḥ pītāḥ śūla-harāḥ param ।।

dravyāṇy etāni pānānne tathā piṇḍopanāhane ।
saha tailaphalair yuñjyāt sāmlāni sneha-vanti ca ।।

sauvarcalāḍhyāṃ madirāṃ piben mūtra-rujāpahām ।
paitte yuñjīta śiśiraṃ seka-lepāvagāhanam ।।

pibed varīṃ gokṣurakaṃ vidārīṃ sa-kaserukām ।
tṛṇākhyaṃ pañca-mūlaṃ ca pākyaṃ sa-madhu-śarkaram ।।

vṛṣakaṃ trapusairvāru-laṭvā-bījāni kuṅkumam ।
drākṣāmbhobhiḥ piban sarvān mūtrāghātān apohati ।।

ervāru-bīja-yaṣṭy-āhva-dārvīr vā taṇḍulāmbunā ।
toyena kalkaṃ drākṣāyāḥ pibet paryuṣitena vā ।।

kapha-je vamanaṃ svedaṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇa-kaṭu-bhojanam ।
yavānāṃ vikṛtīḥ kṣāraṃ kālaśeyaṃ ca śīlayet ।।

piben madyena sūkṣmailāṃ dhātrī-phala-rasena vā ।
sārasāsthi-śvadaṃṣṭrailā-vyoṣaṃ vā madhu-mūtra-vat ।।

sva-rasaṃ kaṇṭakāryā vā pāyayen mākṣikānvitam ।
śitivāraka-bījaṃ vā takreṇa ślakṣṇa-cūrṇitam ।।

dhava-saptāhva-kuṭaja-guḍūcī-caturaṅgulam ।
kembukailā-karañjaṃ ca pākyaṃ sa-madhu sādhitām ।।

aṭukailā-karañjaṃ ca
tair vā peyāṃ pravālaṃ vā cūrṇitaṃ taṇḍulāmbunā ।
sa-tailaṃ pāṭalā-kṣāraṃ sapta-kṛtvo atha-vā srutam ।।

pāṭalī-yāva-śūkābhyāṃ pāribhadrāt tilād api ।
kṣārodakena madirāṃ tvag-eloṣaṇa-saṃyutām ।।

pibed guḍopadaṃśān vā lihyād etān pṛthak pṛthak ।
saṃnipātātmake sarvaṃ yathāvastham idaṃ hitam ।।

aśmany apy a-cirotthāne vāta-vasty-ādikeṣu ca ।
aśmarī dāruṇo vyādhir antaka-pratimo mataḥ ।।

āta-vasty-ādikeṣv api
taruṇo bheṣajaiḥ sādhyaḥ pravṛddhaś chedam arhati ।
tasya pūrveṣu rūpeṣu snehādi-krama iṣyate ।।

pāṣāṇabhedo vasuko vaśiro aśmantako varī ।
kapotavaṅkātibalā-bhallūkośīra-kacchakam ।।

-bhallūkośīra-kantakam
vṛkṣādanī śāka-phalaṃ vyāghryau guṇṭhas trikaṇṭakaḥ ।
yavāḥ kulatthāḥ kolāni varuṇaḥ katakāt phalam ।।

ūṣakādi-pratīvāpam eṣāṃ kvāthe śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।
bhinatti vāta-saṃbhūtāṃ tat pītaṃ śīghram aśmarīm ।।

gandharvahasta-bṛhatī-vyāghrī-gokṣurakekṣurāt ।
mūla-kalkaṃ pibed dadhnā madhureṇāśma-bhedanam ।।

kuśaḥ kāśaḥ śaro guṇṭha itkaṭo moraṭo aśmabhit ।
darbho vidārī vārāhī śāli-mūlaṃ trikaṇṭakaḥ ।।

bhallūkaḥ pāṭalī pāṭhā pattūraḥ sa-kuraṇṭakaḥ ।
punarnave śirīṣaś ca teṣāṃ kvāthe paced ghṛtam ।।

piṣṭena trapusādīnāṃ bījenendīvareṇa ca ।
madhukena śilā-jena tat pittāśmari-bhedanam ।।

varuṇādiḥ samīra-ghnau gaṇāv elā hareṇukā ।
guggulur maricaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ citrakaḥ sa-surāhvayaḥ ।।

taiḥ kalkitaiḥ kṛtāv āpam ūṣakādi-gaṇena ca ।
bhinatti kapha-jām āśu sādhitaṃ ghṛtam aśmarīm ।।

kṣāra-kṣīra-yavāgv-ādi dravyaiḥ svaiḥ svaiś ca kalpayet ।
picukāṅkolla-kataka-śākendīvara-jaiḥ phalaiḥ ।।
