pītam uṣṇāmbu sa-guḍaṃ śarkarā-pātanaṃ param ।
krauñcoṣṭra-rāsabhāsthīni śvadaṃṣṭrā tālapattrikā ।।

ītam uṣṇāmbu sa-ghṛtaṃ
ajamodā kadambasya mūlaṃ viśvasya cauṣadham ।
pītāni śarkarāṃ bhindyuḥ surayoṣṇodakena vā ।।

ūlaṃ bilvasya cauṣadham
nṛtyakuṇḍaka-bījānāṃ cūrṇaṃ mākṣika-saṃyutam ।
avi-kṣīreṇa saptāhaṃ pītam aśmari-pātanaḥ ।।

ṛtyakuṇḍala-bījānāṃ arkaṭakasya bījānāṃ
kvāthaś ca śigru-mūlotthaḥ kad-uṣṇo aśmarī-pātanaḥ ।
tilāpāmārga-kadalī-palāśa-yava-saṃbhavaḥ ।।

kṣāraḥ peyo avi-mūtreṇa śarkarāsv aśmarīṣu ca ।
kapotavaṅkā-mūlaṃ vā pibed ekaṃ surādibhiḥ ।।

tat-siddhaṃ vā pibet kṣīraṃ vedanābhir upadrutaḥ ।
harītaky-asthi-siddhaṃ vā sādhitaṃ vā punarnavaiḥ ।।

kṣīrānna-bhug barhi-śikhā-mūlaṃ vā taṇḍulāmbunā ।
mūtrāghāteṣu vibhajed ataḥ śeṣeṣv api kriyām ।।

bṛhaty-ādi-gaṇe siddhaṃ dvi-guṇī-kṛta-gokṣure ।
toyaṃ payo vā sarpir vā sarva-mūtra-vikāra-jit ।।

devadāruṃ ghanaṃ mūrvāṃ yaṣṭīmadhu harītakīm ।
mūtrāghāteṣu sarveṣu surā-kṣīra-jalaiḥ pibet ।।

rasaṃ vā dhanvayāsasya kaṣāyaṃ kakubhasya vā ।
sukhāmbhasā vā tri-phalāṃ piṣṭāṃ saindhava-saṃyutām ।।

vyāghrī-gokṣuraka-kvāthe yavāgūṃ vā sa-phāṇitām ।
kvāthe vīratarāder vā tāmra-cūḍa-rase api vā ।।

adyād vīratarādyena bhāvitaṃ vā śilā-jatu ।
madyaṃ vā nigadaṃ pītvā rathenāśvena vā vrajet ।।

adyaṃ vā nir-gadaṃ pītvā
śīghra-vegena saṃkṣobhāt tathāsya cyavate aśmarī ।
sarva-thā copayoktavyo vargo vīratarādikaḥ ।।

rekārthaṃ tailvakaṃ sarpir vasti-karma ca śīlayet ।
viśeṣād uttarān vastīñ chukrāśmaryāṃ tu śodhite ।।

hukrāśmaryāṃ ca śodhite
tair mūtra-mārge bala-vān śukrāśaya-viśuddhaye ।
pumān su-tṛpto vṛṣyāṇāṃ māṃsānāṃ kukkuṭasya ca ।।

kāmaṃ sa-kāmaḥ seveta pramadā mada-dāyinīḥ ।
siddhair upakramair ebhir na cec chāntis tadā bhiṣak ।।

a cec chāntis tato bhiṣak
iti rājānam āpṛcchya śastraṃ sādhv avacārayet ।
a-kriyāyāṃ dhruvo mṛtyuḥ kriyāyāṃ saṃśayo bhavet ।।

niścitasyāpi vaidyasya bahu-śaḥ siddha-karmaṇaḥ ।
athāturam upasnigdha-śuddham īṣac ca karśitam ।।

thāturam upasnigdhaṃ -śuddham īṣac ca karṣitam 
śuddham īṣac ca karśitam
abhyakta-svinna-vapuṣam a-bhuktaṃ kṛta-maṅgalam ।
ā-jānu-phalaka-sthasya narasyāṅke vyapāśritam ।।

pūrveṇa kāyenottānaṃ niṣaṇṇaṃ vastra-cumbhale ।
tato asyākuñcite jānu-kūrpare vāsasā dṛḍham ।।

sahāśraya-manuṣyeṇa baddhasyāśvāsitasya ca ।
nābheḥ samantād abhyajyād adhas tasyāś ca vāmataḥ ।।

mṛditvā muṣṭinākrāmed yāvad aśmary adho-gatā ।
tailākte vardhita-nakhe tarjanī-madhyame tataḥ ।।

a-dakṣiṇe gude aṅgulyau praṇidhāyānu-sevani ।
āsādya bala-yatnābhyām aśmarīṃ guda-meḍhrayoḥ ।।

raṇidhāyānu-sevanīm
kṛtvāntare tathā vastiṃ nir-valīkam an-āyatam ।
utpīḍayed aṅgulībhyāṃ yāvad granthir ivonnatam ।।

śalyaṃ syāt sevanīṃ muktvā yava-mātreṇa pāṭayet ।
aśma-mānena na yathā bhidyate sā tathāharet ।।

samagraṃ sarpa-vaktreṇa strīṇāṃ vastis tu pārśva-gaḥ ।
garbhāśayāśrayas tāsāṃ śastram utsaṅga-vat tataḥ ।।

nyased ato anya-thā hy āsāṃ mūtra-srāvī vraṇo bhavet ।
mūtra-praseka-kṣaṇanān narasyāpy api caika-dhā ।।

vasti-bhedo aśmarī-hetuḥ siddhiṃ yāti na tu dvi-dhā ।
vi-śalyam uṣṇa-pānīya-droṇyāṃ tam avagāhayet ।।

tathā na pūryate asreṇa vastiḥ pūrṇe tu pīḍayet ।
meḍhrāntaḥ kṣīri-vṛkṣāmbu mūtra-saṃśuddhaye tataḥ ।।

eḍhrataḥ kṣīri-vṛkṣāmbu eḍhre antaḥ kṣīri-vṛkṣāmbu
kuryād guḍasya sauhityaṃ madhv-ājyākta-vraṇaḥ pibet ।
dvau kālau sa-ghṛtāṃ koṣṇāṃ yavāgūṃ mūtra-śodhanaiḥ ।।

try-ahaṃ daśāhaṃ payasā guḍāḍhyenālpam odanam ।
bhuñjītordhvaṃ phalāmlaiś ca rasair jāṅgala-cāriṇām ।।

kṣīri-vṛkṣa-kaṣāyeṇa vraṇaṃ prakṣālya lepayet ।
prapauṇḍarīka-mañjiṣṭhā-yaṣṭy-āhva-nayanauṣadhaiḥ ।।

vraṇābhyaṅge pacet tailam ebhir eva niśānvitaiḥ ।
daśāhaṃ svedayec cainaṃ sva-mārgaṃ sapta-rātrataḥ ।।

aśāhaṃ svedayec caiva aśāhaṃ svedayec caivaṃ
mūtre tv a-gacchati dahed aśmarī-vraṇam agninā ।
sva-mārga-pratipattau tu svādu-prāyair upācaret ।।

taṃ vastibhir na cārohed varṣaṃ rūḍha-vraṇo api saḥ ।
naga-nāgāśva-vṛkṣa-strī-rathān nāpsu plaveta ca ।।

mūtra-śukra-vahau vasti-vṛṣaṇau sevanīṃ gudam ।
mūtra-prasekaṃ yoniṃ ca śastreṇāṣṭau vivarjayet ।।

cikitsāsthāna
mehino balinaḥ kuryād ādau vamana-recane ।
snigdhasya sarṣapāriṣṭa-nikumbhākṣa-karañja-jaiḥ ।।

tailas trikaṇṭakādyena yathā-svaṃ sādhitena vā ।
snehena musta-devāhva-nāgara-prativāpa-vat ।।

surasādi-kaṣāyeṇa dadyād āsthāpanaṃ tataḥ ।
nyagrodhādes tu pittārtaṃ rasaiḥ śuddhaṃ ca tarpayet ।।

yagrodhādes tu pittārte
mūtra-graha-rujā-gulma-kṣayādyās tv apatarpaṇāt ।
tato anubandha-rakṣārthaṃ śamanāni prayojayet ।।

a-saṃśodhyasya tāny eva sarva-meheṣu pāyayet ।
dhātrī-rasa-plutāṃ prāhṇe haridrāṃ mākṣikānvitām ।।

dārvī-surāhva-tri-phalā-mustā vā kvathitā jale ।
citraka-tri-phalā-dārvī-kaliṅgān vā sa-mākṣikān ।।
madhu-yuktaṃ guḍūcyā vā rasam āmalakasya vā ।।lodhrābhayā-toyada-kaṭphalānāṃ pāṭhā-viḍaṅgārjuna-dhanvanānām ।।gāyatri-dārvī-kṛmihṛd-dhavānāṃ kaphe trayaḥ kṣaudra-yutāḥ kaṣāyāḥ ।।
uśīra-lodhrārjuna-candanānāṃ paṭola-nimbāmalakāmṛtānām ।
lodhrāmbu-kālīyaka-dhātakīnāṃ pitte trayaḥ kṣaudra-yutāḥ kaṣāyāḥ ।।
yathā-svam ebhiḥ pānānnaṃ yava-godhūma-bhāvanāḥ ।।
ava-godhūma-bhāvanām ava-godhūma-bhāvanam
vātolbaṇeṣu snehāṃś ca prameheṣu prakalpayet ।
apūpa-saktu-vāṭyādir yavānāṃ vikṛtir hitā ।।

gajāśva-guda-muktānām atha-vā veṇu-janmanām ।
tṛṇa-dhānyāni mudgādyāḥ śālir jīrṇaḥ sa-ṣaṣṭikaḥ ।।

śrī-kukkuṭo amlaḥ khalakas tila-sarṣapa-kiṭṭa-jaḥ ।
kapitthaṃ tindukaṃ jambūs tat-kṛtā rāga-ṣāḍavāḥ ।।

tiktaṃ śākaṃ madhu śreṣṭhā bhakṣyāḥ śuṣkāḥ sa-saktavaḥ ।
dhanva-māṃsāni śūlyāni pariśuṣkāṇy ayas-kṛtiḥ ।।

madhv-ariṣṭāsavā jīrṇāḥ sīdhuḥ pakva-rasodbhavaḥ ।
tathāsanādi-sārāmbu darbhāmbho mākṣikodakam ।।

vāsiteṣu varā-kvāthe śarvarīṃ śoṣiteṣv ahaḥ ।
yaveṣu su-kṛtān saktūn sa-kṣaudrān sīdhunā pibet ।।

śāla-saptāhva-kampilla-vṛkṣakākṣa-kapittha-jam ।
rohītakaṃ ca kusumaṃ madhunādyāt su-cūrṇitam ।।

kapha-pitta-prameheṣu pibed dhātrī-rasena vā ।
trikaṇṭaka-niśā-lodhra-somavalka-vacārjunaiḥ ।।

padmakāśmantakāriṣṭa-candanāguru-dīpyakaiḥ ।
paṭola-musta-mañjiṣṭhā-mādrī-bhallātakaiḥ pacet ।।

tailaṃ vāta-kaphe pitte ghṛtaṃ miśreṣu miśrakam ।
daśa-mūla-śaṭhī-dantī-surāhvaṃ dvi-punarnavam ।।

mūlaṃ snug-arkayoḥ pathyāṃ bhūkadambam aruṣkaram ।
karañjau varuṇān mūlaṃ pippalyāḥ pauṣkaraṃ ca yat ।।

arañja-varuṇān mūlaṃ
pṛthag daśa-palaṃ prasthān yava-kola-kulatthataḥ ।
trīṃś cāṣṭa-guṇite toye vipacet pāda-vartinā ।।

tena dvi-pippalī-cavya-vacā-nicula-rohiṣaiḥ ।
trivṛd-viḍaṅga-kampilla-bhārgī-viśvaiś ca sādhayet ।।

-bhārgī-bilvaiś ca sādhayet
prasthaṃ ghṛtāj jayet sarvāṃs tan mehān piṭikā viṣam ।
pāṇḍu-vidradhi-gulmārśaḥ-śoṣa-śopha-garodaram ।।

śvāsaṃ kāsaṃ vamiṃ vṛddhiṃ plīhānaṃ vāta-śoṇitam ।
kuṣṭhonmādāv apasmāraṃ dhānvantaram idaṃ ghṛtam ।।

lodhra-mūrvā-śaṭhī-vella-bhārgī-nata-nakha-plavān ।
kaliṅga-kuṣṭha-kramuka-priyaṅgv-ativiṣāgnikān ।।

dve viśāle catur-jātaṃ bhūnimbaṃ kaṭu-rohiṇīm ।
yavānīṃ pauṣkaraṃ pāṭhāṃ granthiṃ cavyaṃ phala-trayam ।।

karṣāṃśam ambu-kalaśe pāda-śeṣe srute hime ।
dvau prasthau mākṣikāt kṣiptvā rakṣet pakṣam upekṣayā ।।

lodhrāsavo ayaṃ mehārśaḥ-śvitra-kuṣṭhā-ruci-kṛmīn ।
pāṇḍu-tvaṃ grahaṇī-doṣaṃ sthūla-tāṃ ca niyacchati ।।

sādhayed asanādīnāṃ palānāṃ viṃśatiṃ pṛthak ।
dvi-vahe apāṃ kṣipet tatra pāda-sthe dve śate guḍāt ।।

kṣaudrāḍhakārdhaṃ palikaṃ vatsakādiṃ ca kalkitam ।
tat kṣaudra-pippalī-cūrṇa-pradigdhe ghṛta-bhājane ।।

atsakādi ca kalkitam
sthitaṃ dṛḍhe jatu-sṛte yava-rāśau nidhāpayet ।
khadirāṅgāra-taptāni bahu-śo atra nimajjayet ।।

tanūni tīkṣṇa-lohasya pattrāṇy ā-loha-saṃkṣayāt ।
ayas-kṛtiḥ sthitā pītā pūrvasmād adhikā guṇaiḥ ।।

rūkṣam udvartanaṃ gāḍhaṃ vyāyāmo niśi jāgaraḥ ।
yac cānyac chleṣma-medo-ghnaṃ bahir antaś ca tad dhitam ।।

su-bhāvitāṃ sāra-jalais tulāṃ pītvā śilodbhavāt ।
sārāmbunaiva bhuñjānaḥ śālīñ jāṅgala-jai rasaiḥ ।।

śāliṃ jāṅgala-jai rasaiḥ
sarvān abhibhaven mehān su-bahūpadravān api ।
gaṇḍa-mālārbuda-granthi-sthaulya-kuṣṭha-bhagandarān ।।

kṛmi-ślīpada-śophāṃś ca paraṃ caitad rasāyanam ।
a-dhanaś chattra-pāda-tra-rahito muni-vartanaḥ ।।

candanam utpalaṃ drākṣā uśīraṃ ca punarnavā ।
yaṣṭīmadhuka-śrīkhaṇḍaṃ tri-phalotpala-śārivā ।।

śamī vaṃśa-phalaṃ lodhraṃ tri-jātaṃ nāgakesaram ।
padmakaṃ ca kaṇā-cūrṇaṃ tat-tulyā śarkarā śubhā ।।

etac cūrṇaṃ pibet prātas taṇḍulodaka-vāriṇā ।
pramehe rakta-pitte ca kṛcchra-doṣe ca dāruṇe ।।

yojanānāṃ śataṃ yāyāt khaned vā salilāśayān ।
go-śakṛn-mūtra-vṛttir vā gobhir eva saha bhramet ।।

bṛṃhayed auṣadhāhārair a-medo-mūtralaiḥ kṛśam ।
śarāvikādyāḥ piṭikāḥ śopha-vat samupācaret ।।

a-pakvā vraṇa-vat pakvās tāsāṃ prāg-rūpam eva ca ।
kṣīri-vṛkṣāmbu pānāya basta-mūtraṃ ca śasyate ।।

tīkṣṇaṃ ca śodhanaṃ prāyo dur-virecyā hi mehinaḥ ।
tailam elādinā kuryād gaṇena vraṇa-ropaṇam ।।

udvartane kaṣāyaṃ tu vargeṇāragvadhādinā ।
pariṣeko asanādyena pānānne vatsakādinā ।।

ariṣeke asanādyena
pāṭhā-citraka-śārṅgaṣṭā-śārivā-kaṇṭakārikāḥ ।
saptāhvaṃ kauṭajaṃ mūlaṃ somavalkaṃ nṛpadrumam ।।

saṃcūrṇya madhunā lihyāt tad-vac cūrṇaṃ navāyasam ।
madhu-mehi-tvam āpanno bhiṣagbhiḥ parivarjitaḥ ।।
śilā-jatu-tulām adyāt pramehārtaḥ punar-navaḥ ।।
cikitsāsthāna
vidradhiṃ sarvam evāmaṃ śopha-vat samupācaret ।
pratataṃ ca hared raktaṃ pakve tu vraṇa-vat kriyā ।।

pañca-mūla-jalair dhautaṃ vātikaṃ lavaṇottaraiḥ ।
bhadrādi-varga-yaṣṭy-āhva-tilair ālepayed vraṇam ।।

vairecanika-yuktena traivṛtena viśodhya ca ।
vidārī-varga-siddhena traivṛtenaiva ropayet ।।

kṣālitaṃ kṣīri-toyena limped yaṣṭy-amṛtā-tilaiḥ ।
paittaṃ ghṛtena siddhena mañjiṣṭhośīra-padmakaiḥ ।।

payasyā-dvi-niśā-śreṣṭhā-yaṣṭī-dugdhaiś ca ropayet ।
nyagrodhādi-pravāla-tvak-phalair vā kapha-jaṃ punaḥ ।।

āragvadhādinā dhautaṃ saktu-kumbha-niśā-tilaiḥ ।
limpet kulatthikā-dantī -trivṛc-chyāmāgni-tilvakaiḥ ।।

āragvadhāmbunā dhautaṃ
sa-saindhavaiḥ sa-go-mūtrais tailaṃ kurvīta ropaṇam ।
raktāgantūdbhave kāryā pitta-vidradhi-vat kriyā ।।

varuṇādi-gaṇa-kvātham a-pakve abhyantarotthite ।
ūṣakādi-pratīvāpaṃ pūrvāhṇe vidradhau pibet ।।

-pakve abhyantara-sthite
ghṛtaṃ virecana-dravyaiḥ siddhaṃ tābhyāṃ ca pāyayet ।
nirūhaṃ sneha-vastiṃ ca tābhyām eva prakalpayet ।।

pāna-bhojana-lepeṣu madhu-śigruḥ prayojitaḥ ।
dattāvāpo yathā-doṣam a-pakvaṃ hanti vidradhim ।।

trāyantī-tri-phalā-nimba-kaṭukā-madhukaṃ samam ।
trivṛt-paṭola-mūlābhyāṃ catvāro aṃśāḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।।

masūrān nis-tuṣād aṣṭau tat-kvāthaḥ sa-ghṛto jayet ।
vidradhi-gulma-vīsarpa-dāha-moha-mada-jvarān ।।

tṛṇ-mūrchā-chardi-hṛd-roga-pittāsṛk-kuṣṭha-kāmalāḥ ।
kuḍavaṃ trāyamāṇāyāḥ sādhyam aṣṭa-guṇe ambhasi ।।

kuḍavaṃ tad-rasād dhātrī-sva-rasāt kṣīrato ghṛtāt ।
karṣāṃśaṃ kalkitaṃ tiktā-trāyantī-dhanvayāsakam ।।

mustā-tāmalakī-vīrā-jīvantī-candanotpalam ।
paced eka-tra saṃyojya tad ghṛtaṃ pūrva-vad guṇaiḥ ।।

drākṣā madhūkaṃ kharjūraṃ vidārī sa-śatāvarī ।
parūṣakāṇi tri-phalā tat-kvāthe pācayed ghṛtam ।।

kṣīrekṣu-dhātrī-niryāsa-prāṇadā-kalka-saṃyutam ।
tac chītaṃ śarkarā-kṣaudra-pādikaṃ pūrva-vad guṇaiḥ ।।

ṣīrekṣu-dhātrī-niryāse rāṇadā-kalka-saṃyutam
harec chṛṅgādibhir asṛk sirayā vā yathāntikam ।
vidradhiṃ pacyamānaṃ ca koṣṭha-sthaṃ bahir-unnatam ।।

jñātvopanāhayet śūle sthite tatraiva piṇḍite ।
tat-pārśva-pīḍanāt suptau dāhādiṣv alpakeṣu ca ।।

pakvaḥ syād vidradhiṃ bhittvā vraṇa-vat tam upācaret ।
antar-bhāgasya cāpy etac cihnaṃ pakvasya vidradeḥ ।।

pakvaḥ srotāṃsi saṃpūrya sa yāty ūrdhvam adho atha-vā ।
svayam-pravṛttaṃ taṃ doṣam upekṣeta hitāśinaḥ ।।

a yāty ūrdhvam adho api vā
daśāhaṃ dvā-daśāhaṃ vā rakṣan bhiṣag upadravāt ।
a-samyag vahati klede varuṇādiṃ sukhāmbhasā ।।

akṣed bhiṣag upadravāt
pāyayen madhu-śigruṃ vā yavāgūṃ tena vā kṛtām ।
yava-kola-kulatthottha-yūṣair annaṃ ca śasyate ।।

ūrdhvaṃ daśāhāt trāyantī-sarpiṣā tailvakena vā ।
śodhayed balataḥ śuddhaḥ sa-kṣaudraṃ tiktakaṃ pibet ।।

sarva-śo gulma-vac cainaṃ yathā-doṣam upācaret ।
sarvāvasthāsu sarvāsu gugguluṃ vidradhīṣu ca ।।

arvāvasthāsu sarveṣu
kaṣāyair yaugikair yuñjyāt svaiḥ svais tad-vac chilā-jatu ।
pākaṃ ca vārayed yatnāt siddhiḥ pakve hi daivikī ।।

api cāśu vidāhi-tvād vidradhiḥ so abhidhīyate ।
sati cālocayen mehe pramehāṇāṃ cikitsitam ।।

śaubhāñjanaka-niryūho hiṅgu-saindhava-saṃyutaḥ ।
a-cirād vidradhiṃ hanti prātaḥ prātar niṣevitaḥ ।।

kaṭu-trikaṃ tiktaka-rohiṇī ghanaṃ kirātatikto atha śatakrator yavāḥ ।
sa-saptaparṇātiviṣā durālabhā paṭola-mūlaṃ saha trāyamāṇayā ।।

guḍūcī-cavyaṃ sa-viḍaṅga-nimbaṃ priyaṅgu-nīlotpala-lodhram añjanam ।
sa-dhātakī-moca-rasaṃ phala-trikaṃ sa-nāgaraṃ bilva-kapittha-śārivāḥ ।।

samāḥ syur ete dvi-guṇaṃ tu citrakaṃ dvir aṣṭa-bhāgaṃ kuṭaja-tvacaṃ syāt ।
su-sūkṣma-piṣṭaṃ śiśirāmbu-yojitaṃ piben manuṣyo ardha-palaṃ guḍānvitam ।।

bubhukṣite syān mṛdu bhojanaṃ hitaṃ śaśaiḥ sa-lāvair atha-vā api tittiraiḥ ।
nihanti gulmān kapha-pitta-saṃbhavān virājate śārada-pūrṇa-candra-vat ।।

a-jīrṇa-kāsaṃ kṣaya-pāṇḍu-te tathā jvarātisāra-grahaṇī-gadāpacīḥ ।
prameha-mūtra-kṣaya-vardhma-vidradhīñ jayet prayuktaḥ sa-guḍaḥ kaṭu-trikaḥ ।। 

।।
bhūnimbārdha-palaṃ niśā-pala-yuktaṃ dārvī-pale dve tathā ।।dārvy-ardhena punarnavāṃ kuru tathā dārvyā samaḥ pragrahaḥ ।।sārdhaṃ duḥsparśataḥ palaṃ tu kaṭukā yojyā tad-ardhena vā ।।aśvāhvaṃ niśayā samānam amṛtā-pādādhikaṃ syāt palam ।।etad vatsaka-sapta-karṣa-sahitaṃ su-ślakṣṇa-cūrṇī-kṛtaṃ ।।vāsāyāḥ sva-rasena pañca caturas trīn vā pibed vāsarān ।।bhūyas tad guḍa-vāriṇā prati-dinaṃ peyaṃ puraḥ-sthe ravau ।।etad vidradhi-rogiṇāṃ ni-ruja-kṛc cūrṇaṃ tu guhyottamam ।।
nā-putrāya na cā-bhrātre nā-śiṣyāyā-hitaiṣiṇe ।
ārogya-śāstra-sarva-svaṃ deyam etat kathañ-ca-na ।।

stana-je vraṇa-vat sarvaṃ na tv enam upanāhayet ।
pāṭayet pālayan stanya-vāhinīḥ kṛṣṇa-cūcukau ।।

sarvāsv āmādy-avasthāsu nirduhīta ca tat stanam ।
śodhayet tri-vṛtā snigdhaṃ vṛddhau snehaiś calātmake ।।

kauśāmra-tilvakairaṇḍa-su-kumāraka-miśrakaiḥ ।
tato anila-ghna-niryūha-kalka-snehair nirūhayet ।।

rasena bhojitaṃ yaṣṭī-tailenānvāsayed anu ।
sveda-pralepā vāta-ghnāḥ pakve bhittvā vraṇa-kriyām ।।

pitta-raktodbhave vṛddhāv āma-pakve yathā-yatham ।
śopha-vraṇa-kriyāṃ kuryāt pratataṃ ca hared asṛk ।।

go-mūtreṇa pibet kalkaṃ ślaiṣmike pītadāru-jam ।
vimlāpanād ṛte cāsya śleṣma-granthi-kramo hitaḥ ।।

imlāpanād ṛte cātra
pakve ca pāṭite tailam iṣyate vraṇa-śodhanam ।
sumano-'ruṣkarāṅkolla-saptaparṇeṣu sādhitam ।।

paṭola-nimba-rajanī-viḍaṅga-kuṭajeṣu ca ।
medo-jaṃ mūtra-piṣṭena su-svinnaṃ surasādinā ।।

śiro-vireka-dravyair vā varjayan phala-sevanīm ।
dārayed vṛddhi-pattreṇa samyaṅ medasi sūddhṛte ।।

amyaṅ medasi coddhṛte
vraṇaṃ mākṣika-kāsīsa-saindhava-pratisāritam ।
sīvyed abhyañjanaṃ cāsya yojyaṃ medo-viśuddhaye ।।

manaḥśilailā-sumano-granthi-bhallātakaiḥ kṛtam ।
tailam ā-vraṇa-saṃdhānāt sneha-svedau ca śīlayet ।।

mūtra-jaṃ sveditaṃ snigdhair vastra-paṭṭena veṣṭitam ।
vidhyed adhas-tāt sevanyāḥ srāvayec ca yathodaram ।।

vraṇaṃ ca sthagikā-baddhaṃ ropayed antra-hetuke ।
phala-kośam a-saṃprāpte cikitsā vāta-vṛddhi-vat ।।

pacet punarnava-tulāṃ tathā daśa-palāḥ pṛthak ।
daśa-mūla-payasyāśvagandhairaṇḍa-śatāvarīḥ ।।

dvi-darbha-śara-kāśekṣu-mūla-poṭagalānvitāḥ ।
vahe apām aṣṭa-bhāga-sthe tatra triṃśat-palaṃ guḍāt ।।

prastham eraṇḍa-tailasya dvau ghṛtāt payasas tathā ।
āvaped dvi-palāṃśaṃ ca kṛṣṇā-tan-mūla-saindhavam ।।

yaṣṭīmadhuka-mṛdvīkā-yavānī-nāgarāṇi ca ।
tat-siddhaṃ su-kumārākhyaṃ su-kumāraṃ rasāyanam ।।

vātātapādhva-yānādi-parihāryeṣv a-yantraṇam ।
prayojyaṃ su-kumārāṇām īśvarāṇām sukhātmanām ।।

nṛṇāṃ strī-vṛnda-bhartṝṇām a-lakṣmī-kali-nāśanam ।
sarva-kālopayogena kānti-lāvaṇya-puṣṭi-dam ।।

vardhma-vidradhi-gulmārśo-yoni-meḍhrānilārtiṣu ।
śophodara-khuḍa-plīha-viḍ-vibandheṣu cottamam ।।

rāsnā-yaṣṭy-amṛtairaṇḍa-balā-gokṣura-sādhitaḥ ।
kvātho antra-vṛddhiṃ hanty āśu rubu-tailena miśritaḥ ।।

yāyād vardhma na cec chāntiṃ sneha-rekānuvāsanaiḥ ।
vasti-karma puraḥ kṛtvā vaṅkṣaṇa-sthaṃ tato dahet ।।

agninā mārga-rodhārthaṃ maruto ardhendu-vakrayā ।
aṅguṣṭhasyopari snāva pītaṃ tantu-samaṃ ca yat ।।

utkṣipya sūcyā tat tiryag dahec chittvā yato gadaḥ ।
tato anya-pārśve anye tv āhur dahed vānāmikāṅguleḥ ।।

gulme anyair vāta-kapha-je plīhni cāyaṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।
kaniṣṭhikānāmikayor viśvācyāṃ ca yato gadaḥ ।।
mūlaṃ bilva-kapitthayoḥ aralukasyāgner bṛhatyor dvayoḥ ।।śyāmā-pūti-karañja-śigruka-taror viśvauṣadhāruṣkaram ।।kṛṣṇā-granthika-vella-pañca-lavaṇa-kṣārājamodānvitaṃ ।।pītaṃ kāñjika-toyamathitaiś cūrṇī-kṛtaṃ vardhma-jit ।।
ajājī-kuṣṭha-gomeda-hapuṣā-badarāṇi ca ।
āranālena lepaḥ syād vardhma-jit param auṣadham ।।

avi-kṣīreṇa godhūma-cūrṇaṃ kandurukasya ca ।
pralepanaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ syād vardhma-jit param auṣadham ।।

mṛta-mātre tu vai kāke viśastena pralepayet ।
muhūrtaṃ vardhma medhāvī tat-kṣaṇād a-rujo bhavet ।।

cikitsāsthāna
gulmaṃ baddha-śakṛd-vātaṃ vātikaṃ tīvra-vedanam ।
rūkṣa-śītodbhavaṃ tailaiḥ sādhayed vāta-rogikaiḥ ।।

pānānnānvāsanābhyaṅgaiḥ snigdhasya svedam ācaret ।
ānāha-vedanā-stambha-vibandheṣu viśeṣataḥ ।।

srotasāṃ mārdavaṃ kṛtvā jitvā mārutam ulbaṇam ।
bhittvā vibandhaṃ snigdhasya svedo gulmam apohati ।।

sneha-pānaṃ hitaṃ gulme viśeṣeṇordhva-nābhi-je ।
pakvāśaya-gate vastir ubhayaṃ jaṭharāśraye ।।

dīpte agnau vātike gulme vibandhe anila-varcasoḥ ।
bṛṃhaṇāny anna-pānāni snigdhoṣṇāni pradāpayet ।।

punaḥ punaḥ sneha-pānaṃ nirūhāḥ sānuvāsanāḥ ।
prayojyā vāta-je gulme kapha-pittānurakṣiṇaḥ ।।

apha-pittānurakṣiṇā
vasti-karma paraṃ vidyād gulma-ghnaṃ tad dhi mārutam ।
sva-sthāne prathamaṃ jitvā sadyo gulmam apohati ।।

tasmād abhīkṣṇa-śo gulmā nirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ ।
prayujyamānaiḥ śāmyanti vāta-pitta-kaphātmakāḥ ।।

hiṅgu-sauvarcala-vyoṣa-viḍa-dāḍima-dīpyakaiḥ ।
puṣkarājājī-dhānyāmla-vetasa-kṣāra-citrakaiḥ ।।

śaṭhī-vacājagandhailā-surasair dadhi-saṃyutaiḥ ।
śūlānāha-haraṃ sarpiḥ sādhayed vāta-gulminām ।।

hapuṣoṣaṇa-pṛthvīkā-pañca-kolaka-dīpyakaiḥ ।
sājājī-saindhavair dadhnā dugdhena ca rasena ca ।।

dāḍimān mūlakāt kolāt pacet sarpir nihanti tat ।
vāta-gulmodarānāha-pārśva-hṛt-koṣṭha-vedanāḥ ।।

yony-arśo-grahaṇī-doṣa-kāsa-śvāsā-ruci-jvarān ।
daśa-mūlaṃ balāṃ kālāṃ suṣavīṃ dvau punarnavau ।।

aśa-mūlaṃ balāṃ kālīṃ
pauṣkarairaṇḍa-rāsnāśvagandhā-bhārgy-amṛtā-śaṭhīḥ ।
paced gandha-palāśaṃ ca droṇe apāṃ dvi-palonmitam ।।

yavaiḥ kolaiḥ kulatthaiś ca māṣaiś ca prāsthikaiḥ saha ।
kvāthe asmin dadhi-pātre ca ghṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।।

sva-rasair dāḍimāmrāta-mātuluṅgodbhavair yutam ।
tathā tuṣāmbu-dhānyāmla-śuktaiḥ ślakṣṇaiś ca kalkitaiḥ ।।

bhārgī-tumburu-ṣaḍgranthā-granthi-rāsnāgni-dhānyakaiḥ ।
yavānaka-yavāny-amla-vetasāsita-jīrakaiḥ ।।

ajājī-hiṅgu-hapuṣā-kāravī-vṛṣakoṣakaiḥ ।
nikumbha-kumbha-mūrvebha-pippalī-vella-dāḍimaiḥ ।।

śvadaṃṣṭrā-trapusairvāru-bīja-hiṃsrāśmabhedakaiḥ ।
miśi-dvi-kṣāra-surasa-śārivā-nīlinī-phalaiḥ ।।

tri-kaṭu-tri-paṭūpetair dādhikaṃ tad vyapohati ।
rogān āśu-tarān pūrvān kaṣṭān api ca śīlitam ।।

apasmāra-gadonmāda-mūtrāghātānilāmayān ।
try-ūṣaṇa-tri-phalā-dhānya-cavikā-vella-citrakaiḥ ।।

pasmāra-garonmāda-
kalkī-kṛtair ghṛtaṃ pakvaṃ sa-kṣīraṃ vāta-gulma-nut ।
tulāṃ laśuna-kandānāṃ pṛthak pañca-palāṃśakam ।।

pañca-mūlaṃ mahac cāmbu-bhārārdhe tad vipācayet ।
pāda-śeṣaṃ tad-ardhena dāḍima-sva-rasaṃ surām ।।

dhānyāmlaṃ dadhi cādāya piṣṭāṃś cārdha-palāṃśakān ।
try-ūṣaṇa-tri-phalā-hiṅgu-yavānī-cavya-dīpyakān ।।

sāmla-vetasa-sindhūttha-devadārūn paced ghṛtāt ।
taiḥ prasthaṃ tat paraṃ sarva-vāta-gulma-vikāra-jit ।।

āmla-vetasa-sindhūtthaṃ evadāru paced ghṛtāt
ṣaṭ-palaṃ vā pibet sarpir yad uktaṃ rāja-yakṣmaṇi ।
prasannayā vā kṣīrārthaḥ surayā dāḍimena vā ।।

ghṛte māruta-gulma-ghnaḥ kāryo dadhnaḥ sareṇa vā ।
vāta-gulme kapho vṛddho hatvāgnim a-ruciṃ yadi ।।

hṛl-lāsaṃ gauravaṃ tandrāṃ janayed ullikhet tu tam ।
śūlānāha-vibandheṣu jñātvā sa-sneham āśayam ।।

niryūha-cūrṇa-vaṭakāḥ prayojyā ghṛta-bheṣajaiḥ ।
kola-dāḍima-gharmāmbu-takra-madyāmla-kāñjikaih ।।

maṇḍena vā pibet prātaś cūrṇāny annasya vā puraḥ ।
cūrṇāni mātuluṅgasya bhāvitāny a-sakṛd rase ।।
kurvīta kārmuka-tarān vaṭakān kapha-vātayoḥ ।।hiṅgu-vacā-vijayā-paśugandhā-dāḍima-dīpyaka-dhānyaka-pāṭhāḥ ।।puṣkara-mūla-śaṭhī-hapuṣāgni-kṣāra-yuga-tri-paṭu-tri-kaṭūni ।।
sājāji-cavyaṃ saha-tintiḍīkaṃ sa-vetasāmlaṃ vinihanti cūrṇaṃ ।
hṛt-pārśva-vasti-trika-yoni-pāyu-śūlāni vāyv-āma-kaphodbhavāni ।।

kṛcchrān gulmān vāta-viṇ-mūtra-saṅgaṃ kaṇṭhe bandhaṃ hṛd-grahaṃ pāṇḍu-rogam ।
annā-śraddhā-plīha-dur-nāma-hidhmā-vardhmādhmāna-śvāsa-kāsāgni-sādān ।।

lavaṇa-yavānī-dīpyaka-kaṇa-nāgaram uttarottaraṃ vṛddham ।
sarva-samāṃśa-harītakī- cūrṇaṃ vaiśvānaraḥ sākṣāt ।।

arva-samāṃśaṃ harītakī- arva-samāṃśā vijayā- v
cūrṇo vaiśvānaraḥ sākṣāt
tri-kaṭukam ajamodā saindhavaṃ jīrake dve ।।
sama-dharaṇa-ghṛtānām aṣṭamo hiṅgu-bhāgaḥ ।।prathama-kavaḍa-bhojyaḥ sarpiṣā saṃprayukto ।।
rathama-kavaḍa-bhojyaḥ sarpiṣā cūrṇako ayaṃ janayati jaṭharāgniṃ vāta-gulmaṃ nihanti ।।

anayati bhṛśam agniṃ vāta-gulmaṃ nihanti hiṅgūgrā-viḍa-śuṇṭhy-ajāji-vijayā-vāṭyābhidhānāmayaiś ।।
cūrṇaḥ kumbha-nikumbha-mūla-sahitair bhāgottaraṃ vardhitaiḥ ।।pītaḥ koṣṇa-jalena koṣṭha-ja-rujo gulmodarādīn ayaṃ ।।śārdūlaḥ prasabhaṃ pramathya harati vyādhīn mṛgaughān iva ।।sindhūttha-pathyā-kaṇa-dīpyakānāṃ ।।cūrṇāni toyaiḥ pibatāṃ kavoṣṇaiḥ ।।prayāti nāśaṃ kapha-vāta-janmā ।।nārāca-nirbhinna ivāmayaughaḥ ।।pūtīka-pattra-gaja-cirbhaṭa-cavya-vahni- ।।-vyoṣaṃ ca saṃstara-citaṃ lavaṇopadhānam ।।dagdhvā vicūrṇya dadhi-mastu-yutaṃ prayojyaṃ ।।gulmodara-śvayathu-pāṇḍu-gudodbhaveṣu ।।
ulmodara-śvayathu-pāṇḍu-gadodbhaveṣu hiṅgu-tri-guṇaṃ saindhavam asmāt tri-guṇaṃ ca tailam airaṇḍam ।।

tat tri-guṇa-laśuna-rasaṃ gulmodara-vardhma-śūla-ghnam ।
mātuluṅga-raso hiṅgu dāḍimaṃ viḍa-saindhavam ।।

surā-maṇḍena pātavyaṃ vāta-gulma-rujāpaham ।
śuṇṭhyāḥ karṣaṃ guḍasya dvau dhautāt kṛṣṇa-tilāt palam ।।

āta-gulma-jvarāpaham
khādann eka-tra saṃcūrṇya koṣṇa-kṣīrānupo jayet ।
vāta-hṛd-roga-gulmārśo-yoni-śūla-śakṛd-grahān ।।

pibed eraṇḍa-tailaṃ tu vāta-gulmī prasannayā ।
śleṣmaṇy anu-bale vāyau pitte tu payasā saha ।।

vivṛddhaṃ yadi vā pittaṃ saṃtāpaṃ vāta-gulminaḥ ।
kuryād virecanīyo asau sa-snehair ānulomikaiḥ ।।

tāpānuvṛttāv evaṃ ca raktaṃ tasyāvasecayet ।
sādhayec chuddha-śuṣkasya laśunasya catuḥ-palam ।।

kṣīrodake aṣṭa-guṇite kṣīra-śeṣaṃ ca pācayet ।
vāta-gulmam udāvartaṃ gṛdhrasīṃ viṣama-jvaram ।।

hṛd-rogaṃ vidradhiṃ śoṣaṃ sādhayaty āśu tat payaḥ ।
tailaṃ prasannā go-mūtram āranālaṃ yavāgra-jaḥ ।।

āśayaty āśu tat payaḥ
gulmaṃ jaṭharam ānāhaṃ pītam eka-tra sādhayet ।
citraka-granthikairaṇḍa-śuṇṭhī-kvāthaḥ paraṃ hitaḥ ।।

śūlānāha-vibandheṣu sa-hiṅgu-viḍa-saindhavaiḥ ।
puṣkarairaṇḍayor mūlaṃ yava-dhanvayavāsakam ।।

jalena kvathitaṃ pītaṃ koṣṭha-dāha-rujāpaham ।
vāṭyāhvairaṇḍa-darbhāṇāṃ mūlaṃ dāru mahauṣadham ।।

pītaṃ niḥkvāthya toyena koṣṭha-pṛṣṭhāṃsa-śūla-jit ।
śilā-jaṃ payasān-alpa-pañca-mūla-śṛtena vā ।।

oṣṭha-pṛṣṭy-aṃsa-śūla-jit
vāta-gulmī pibed vāṭyam udāvarte tu bhojayet ।
snigdhaṃ paippalikair yūṣair mūlakānāṃ rasena vā ।।

baddha-viṇ-māruto aśnīyāt kṣīreṇoṣṇena yāvakam ।
kulmāṣān vā bahu-snehān bhakṣayel lavaṇottarān ।।

nīlinī-trivṛtā-dantī-pathyā-kampillakaiḥ saha ।
sa-malāya ghṛtaṃ deyaṃ sa-viḍa-kṣāra-nāgaram ।।

nīlinīṃ tri-phalāṃ rāsnāṃ balāṃ kaṭuka-rohiṇīm ।
paced viḍaṅgaṃ vyāghrīṃ ca pālikāni jalāḍhake ।।

rase aṣṭa-bhāga-śeṣe tu ghṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।
dadhnaḥ prasthena saṃyojya sudhā-kṣīra-palena ca ।।

tato ghṛta-palaṃ dadyād yavāgū-maṇḍa-miśritam ।
jīrṇe samyag-viriktaṃ ca bhojayed rasa-bhojanam ।।

gulma-kuṣṭhodara-vyaṅga-śopha-pāṇḍv-āmaya-jvarān ।
śvitraṃ plīhānam unmādaṃ hanty etan nīlinī-ghṛtam ।।

kukkuṭāś ca mayūrāś ca tittiri-krauñca-vartakāḥ ।
śālayo madirā sarpir vāta-gulma-cikitsitam ।।

mitam uṣṇaṃ dravaṃ snigdhaṃ bhojanaṃ vāta-gulminām ।
sa-maṇḍā vāruṇī pānaṃ taptaṃ vā dhānyakair jalam ।।

snigdhoṣṇenodite gulme paittike sraṃsanaṃ hitam ।
drākṣābhayā-guḍa-rasaṃ kampillaṃ vā madhu-drutam ।।

ampillaṃ vā madhu-dravam
kalpoktaṃ rakta-pittoktaṃ gulme rūkṣoṣṇa-je punaḥ ।
paraṃ saṃśamanaṃ sarpis tiktaṃ vāsā-ghṛtaṃ śṛtam ।।

tṛṇākhya-pañcaka-kvāthe jīvanīya-gaṇena vā ।
śṛtaṃ tenaiva vā kṣīraṃ nyagrodhādi-gaṇena vā ।।

tatrāpi sraṃsanaṃ yuñjyāc chīghram ātyayike bhiṣak ।
vairecanika-siddhena sarpiṣā payasāpi vā ।।

rasenāmalakekṣūṇāṃ ghṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।
pathyā-pādaṃ pibet sarpis tat siddhaṃ pitta-gulma-nut ।।

pibed vā tailvakaṃ sarpir yac coktaṃ pitta-vidradhau ।
drākṣāṃ payasyāṃ madhukaṃ candanaṃ padmakaṃ madhu ।।

pibet taṇḍula-toyena pitta-gulmopaśāntaye ।
dvi-palaṃ trāyamāṇāyā jala-dvi-prastha-sādhitam ।।

aṣṭa-bhāga-sthitaṃ pūtaṃ koṣṇaṃ kṣīra-samam pibet ।
pibed upari tasyoṣṇaṃ kṣīram eva yathā-balam ।।

tena nirhṛta-doṣasya gulmaḥ śāmyati paittikaḥ ।
dāhe abhyaṅgo ghṛtaiḥ śītaiḥ sājyair lepo himauṣadhaiḥ ।।

sparśaḥ saro-ruhāṃ pattraiḥ pātraiś ca pracalaj-jalaiḥ ।
vidāha-pūrva-rūpeṣu śūle vahneś ca mārdave ।।

bahu-śo apahared raktaṃ pitta-gulme viśeṣataḥ ।
chinna-mūlā vidahyante na gulmā yānti ca kṣayam ।।

raktaṃ hi vy-amla-tāṃ yāti tac ca nāsti na cāsti ruk ।
hṛta-doṣaṃ parimlānaṃ jāṅgalais tarpitaṃ rasaiḥ ।।

samāśvastaṃ sa-śeṣārtiṃ sarpir abhyāsayet punaḥ ।
rakta-pittāti-vṛddha-tvāt kriyām an-upalabhya vā ।।

gulme pākon-mukhe sarvā pitta-vidradhi-vat kriyā ।
śālir gavyāja-payasī paṭolī jāṅgalaṃ ghṛtam ।।

dhātrī parūṣakaṃ drākṣā kharjūraṃ dāḍimaṃ sitā ।
bhojyaṃ pāne ambu balayā bṛhaty-ādyaiś ca sādhitam ।।

śleṣma-je vāmayet pūrvam a-vamyam upavāsayet ।
tiktoṣṇa-kaṭu-saṃsargyā vahniṃ saṃdhukṣayet tataḥ ।।

apha-je vāmayet pūrvam
hiṅgv-ādibhiś ca dvi-guṇa-kṣāra-hiṅgv-amla-vetasaiḥ ।
nigūḍhaṃ yadi vonnaddhaṃ stimitaṃ kaṭhinaṃ sthiram ।।

ānāhādi-yutaṃ gulmaṃ saṃsvedya vinayed anu ।
ghṛtaṃ sa-kṣāra-kaṭukaṃ pātavyaṃ kapha-gulminām ।।

aṃśodhya vinayed anu
sa-vyoṣa-kṣāra-lavaṇaṃ sa-hiṅgu-viḍa-dāḍimam ।
kapha-gulmaṃ jayaty āśu daśa-mūla-śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।।

bhallātakānāṃ dvi-palaṃ pañca-mūlaṃ palonmitam ।
alpaṃ toyāḍhake sādhyaṃ pāda-śeṣeṇa tena ca ।।

tulyaṃ ghṛtaṃ tulya-payo vipaced akṣa-saṃmitaiḥ ।
viḍaṅga-hiṅgu-sindhūttha-yāva-śūka-śaṭhī-viḍaiḥ ।।

sa-dvīpi-rāsnā-yaṣṭy-āhva-ṣaḍgranthā-kaṇa-nāgaraiḥ ।
etad bhallātaka-ghṛtaṃ kapha-gulma-haraṃ param ।।

plīha-pāṇḍv-āmaya-śvāsa-grahaṇī-roga-kāsa-jit ।
tato asya gulme dehe ca samaste svedam ācaret ।।

-grahaṇī-roga-kāsa-nut
sarva-tra gulme prathamaṃ sneha-svedopapādite ।
yā kriyā kriyate yāti sā siddhiṃ na virūkṣite ।।

snigdha-svinna-śarīrasya gulme śaithilyam āgate ।
yathoktāṃ ghaṭikāṃ nyasyed gṛhīte apanayec ca tām ।।

vastrāntaraṃ tataḥ kṛtvā bhindyād gulmaṃ pramāṇa-vit ।
vi-mārgāja-padādarśair yathā-lābhaṃ prapīḍayet ।।

pramṛjyād gulmam evaikaṃ na tv antra-hṛdayaṃ spṛśet ।
tilairaṇḍātasī-bīja-sarṣapaiḥ parilipya ca ।।

-sarṣapaiḥ parilipya vā
śleṣma-gulmam ayaḥ-pātraiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ svedayet tataḥ ।
evaṃ ca visṛtaṃ sthānāt kapha-gulmaṃ virecanaiḥ ।।

sa-snehair vastibhiś cainaṃ śodhayed dāśamūlikaiḥ ।
pippaly-āmalaka-drākṣā-śyāmādyaiḥ pālikaiḥ pacet ।।

eraṇḍa-taila-haviṣoḥ prasthau payasi ṣaḍ-guṇe ।
siddho ayaṃ miśrakaḥ sneho gulmināṃ sraṃsanaṃ hitam ।।

vṛddhi-vidradhi-śūleṣu vāta-vyādhiṣu cāmṛtam ।
pibed vā nīlinī-sarpir mātrayā dvi-palīnayā ।।

ātrayā dvi-palīkayā
tathaiva su-kumārākhyaṃ ghṛtāny audarikāṇi vā ।
droṇe ambhasaḥ paced dantyāḥ palānāṃ pañca-viṃśatim ।।

citrakasya tathā pathyās tāvatīs tad-rase srute ।
dvi-prasthe sādhayet pūte kṣiped dantī-samaṃ guḍam ।।

āvatīs tad-rase śṛte
tailāt palāni catvāri trivṛtāyaś ca cūrṇataḥ ।
kaṇā-karṣau tathā śuṇṭhyāḥ siddhe lehe tu śītale ।।

madhu taila-samaṃ dadyāc catur-jātāc caturthikām ।
ato harītakīm ekāṃ sāvaleha-palām adan ।।

sukhaṃ viricyate snigdho doṣa-prastham an-āmayaḥ ।
gulma-hṛd-roga-dur-nāma-śophānāha-garodarān ।।

kuṣṭhotkleśā-ruci-plīha-grahaṇī-viṣama-jvarān ।
ghnanti dantī-harītakyaḥ pāṇḍu-tāṃ ca sa-kāmalām ।।

āṇḍu-tāṃ ca sa-kāmalān
sudhā-kṣīra-dravaṃ cūrṇaṃ tri-vṛtāyāḥ su-bhāvitam ।
kārṣikaṃ madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ līḍhvā sādhu viricyate ।।

kuṣṭha-śyāmā-trivṛd-dantī-vijayā-kṣāra-guggulūn ।
go-mūtreṇa pibed ekaṃ tena guggulum eva vā ।।

nirūhān kalpa-siddhy-uktān yojayed gulma-nāśanān ।
kṛta-mūlaṃ mahā-vāstuṃ kaṭhinaṃ stimitaṃ gurum ।।

gūḍha-māṃsaṃ jayed gulmaṃ kṣārāriṣṭāgni-karmabhiḥ ।
ekāntaram dvy-antaraṃ vā viśramayyātha-vā try-aham ।।

śarīra-doṣa-balayor vardhana-kṣapaṇodyataḥ ।
arśo-'śmarī-grahaṇy-uktāḥ kṣārā yojyāḥ kapholbaṇe ।।

devadāru-trivṛd-dantī-kaṭukā-pañca-kolakam ।
svarjikā-yāva-śūkākhyau śreṣṭhā-pāṭhopakuñcikāḥ ।।

kuṣṭhaṃ sarpasugandhāṃ ca dvy-akṣāṃśaṃ paṭu-pañcakam ।
pālikaṃ cūrṇitaṃ taila-vasā-dadhi-ghṛtāplutam ।।

ghaṭasyāntaḥ pacet pakvam agni-varṇe ghaṭe ca tam ।
kṣāraṃ gṛhītvā kṣīrājya-takra-madyādibhiḥ pibet ।।

gulmodāvarta-vardhmārśo-jaṭhara-grahaṇī-kṛmīn ।
apasmāra-garonmāda-yoni-śukrāmayāśmarīḥ ।।

kṣārā-gado ayaṃ śamayed viṣaṃ cākhu-bhujaṅga-jam ।
śleṣmāṇaṃ madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ rasa-kṣīra-ghṛtāśinaḥ ।।

chittvā bhittvāśayāt kṣāraḥ kṣāra-tvāt kṣārayaty adhaḥ ।
mande agnāv a-rucau sātmyair madyaiḥ sa-sneham aśnatām ।।

hittvā chittvāśayāt kṣāraḥ hittvā bhittvāśayaṃ kṣāraḥ 
ṣāra-tvāt pātayaty adhaḥ
yojayed āsavāriṣṭān nigadān mārga-śuddhaye ।
śālayaḥ ṣaṣṭikā jīrṇāḥ kulatthā jāṅgalaṃ palam ।।

ciribilvāgni-tarkārī-yavānī-varuṇāṅkurāḥ ।
śigrus taruṇa-bilvāni bālaṃ śuṣkaṃ ca mūlakam ।।

śigros taruṇa-mūlāni
bījapūraka-hiṅgv-amla-vetasa-kṣāra-dāḍimam ।
vyoṣaṃ takraṃ ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ bhaktaṃ pānaṃ tu vāruṇī ।।

dhānyāmlaṃ mastu takraṃ ca yavānī-viḍa-cūrṇitam ।
pañca-mūla-śṛtaṃ vāri jīrṇaṃ mārdvīkam eva vā ।।

pippalī-pippalī-mūla-citrakājājī-saindhavaiḥ ।
surā gulmaṃ jayaty āśu jagalaś ca vimiśritaḥ ।।

āṅgalaś ca vimiśritaḥ
vamanair laṅghanaiḥ svedaiḥ sarpiḥ-pānair virecanaiḥ ।
vasti-kṣārāsavāriṣṭa-guṭikā-pathya-bhojanaiḥ ।।

asti-kṣārāsavāriṣṭair -gulmikā-pathya-bhojanaiḥ 
gaulmikaiḥ pathya-bhojanaiḥ
ślaiṣmiko baddha-mūla-tvād yadi gulmo na śāmyati ।
tasya dāhaṃ hṛte rakte kuryād ante śarādibhiḥ ।।

atha gulmaṃ sa-pary-antaṃ vāsasāntaritaṃ bhiṣak ।
nābhi-vasty-antra-hṛdayaṃ roma-rājīṃ ca varjayan ।।

nāti-gāḍhaṃ parimṛśec chareṇa jvalatātha-vā ।
lohenāraṇikotthena dāruṇā taindukena vā ।।

tato agni-vege śamite śītair vraṇa iva kriyā ।
āmānvaye tu peyādyaiḥ saṃdhukṣyāgniṃ vilaṅghite ।।

svaṃ svaṃ kuryāt kramaṃ miśraṃ miśra-doṣe ca kāla-vit ।
gata-prasava-kālāyai nāryai gulme asra-saṃbhave ।।

snigdha-svinna-śarīrāyai dadyāt sneha-virecanam ।
tila-kvāthe ghṛta-guḍa-vyoṣa-bhārgī-rajo-'nvitaḥ ।।

pānaṃ rakta-bhave gulme naṣṭe puṣpe ca yoṣitaḥ ।
bhārgī-kṛṣṇā-karañja-tvag-granthikāmaradāru-jam ।।

cūrṇaṃ tilānāṃ kvāthena pītaṃ gulma-rujāpaham ।
palāśa-kṣāra-pātre dve dve pātre taila-sarpiṣoḥ ।।

gulma-śaithilya-jananīṃ paktvā mātrāṃ prayojayet ।
na prabhidyeta yady evaṃ dadyād yoni-virecanam ।।

kṣāreṇa yuktaṃ palalaṃ sudhā-kṣīreṇa vā tataḥ ।
tābhyāṃ vā bhāvitān dadyād yonau kaṭuka-matsyakān ।।

varāha-matsya-pittābhyāṃ naktakān vā su-bhāvitān ।
kiṇvaṃ vā sa-guḍa-kṣāraṃ dadyād yonau viśuddhaye ।।

rakta-pitta-haraṃ kṣāraṃ lehayen madhu-sarpiṣā ।
laśunaṃ madirāṃ tīkṣṇāṃ matsyāṃś cāsyai prayojayet ।।

vastiṃ sa-kṣīra-go-mūtraṃ sa-kṣāraṃ dāśamūlikam ।
a-vartamāne rudhire hitaṃ gulma-prabhedanam ।।

astiṃ sa-kṣaudra-go-mutraṃ
yamakābhyakta-dehāyāḥ pravṛtte samupekṣaṇam ।
rasaudanas tathāhāraḥ pānaṃ ca taruṇī surā ।।

rudhire ati-pravṛtte tu rakta-pitta-harāḥ kriyāḥ ।
kāryā vāta-rug-ārtāyāḥ sarvā vāta-harāḥ punaḥ ।।
ānāhādāv udāvarta-balāsa-ghnyo yathā-yatham ।।
cikitsāsthāna
doṣāti-mātropacayāt sroto-mārga-nirodhanāt ।
saṃbhavaty udaraṃ tasmān nityam enaṃ virecayet ।।

roto-mārga-vighātanāt
pāyayet tailam airaṇḍaṃ sa-mūtraṃ sa-payo api vā ।
māsaṃ dvau vātha-vā gavyaṃ mūtraṃ māhiṣam eva vā ।।

āsaṃ dvau vā tathā gavyaṃ
pibed go-kṣīra-bhuk syād vā karabhī-kṣīra-vartanaḥ ।
dāhānāhāti-tṛṇ-mūrchā-parītas tu viśeṣataḥ ।।

rūkṣāṇāṃ bahu-vātānāṃ doṣa-saṃśuddhi-kāṅkṣiṇām ।
snehanīyāni sarpīṃṣi jaṭhara-ghnāni yojayet ।।

ṣaṭ-palaṃ daśa-mūlāmbu-mastu-dvy-āḍhaka-sādhitam ।
nāgara-tri-palaṃ prasthaṃ ghṛta-tailāt tathāḍhakam ।।

āgaraṃ tri-palaṃ prasthaṃ
mastunaḥ sādhayitvaitat pibet sarvodarāpaham ।
kapha-māruta-saṃbhūte gulme ca paramaṃ hitam ।।

catur-guṇe jale mūtre dvi-guṇe citrakāt pale ।
kalke siddhaṃ ghṛta-prasthaṃ sa-kṣāraṃ jaṭharī pibet ।।

yava-kola-kulatthānāṃ pañca-mūlasya cāmbhasā ।
surā-sauvīrakābhyāṃ ca siddhaṃ vā pāyayed ghṛtam ।।

ebhiḥ snigdhāya saṃjāte bale śānte ca mārute ।
sraste doṣāśaye dadyāt kalpa-dṛṣṭaṃ virecanam ।।

paṭola-mūlaṃ tri-phalāṃ niśāṃ vellaṃ ca kārṣikam ।
kampilla-nīlinī-kumbha-bhāgān dvi-tri-catur-guṇān ।।

pibet saṃcūrṇya mūtreṇa peyā-pūrvaṃ tato rasaiḥ ।
virikto jāṅgalair adyāt tataḥ ṣaḍ-divasaṃ payaḥ ।।

śṛtaṃ pibed vyoṣa-yutaṃ pītam evaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।
hanti sarvodarāṇy etac cūrṇaṃ jātodakāny api ।।

gavākṣīṃ śaṅkhinīṃ dantīṃ tilvakasya tvacaṃ vacām ।
pibet karkandhu-mṛdvīkā-kolāmbho-mūtra-sīdhubhiḥ ।।

yavānī hapuṣā dhānyaṃ śatapuṣpopakuñcikā ।
kāravī pippalī-mūlam ajagandhā śaṭhī vacā ।।

citrako ajājikaṃ vyoṣaṃ svarṇakṣīrī phala-trayam ।
dvau kṣārau pauṣkaraṃ mūlaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ lavaṇa-pañcakam ।।

viḍaṅgaṃ ca samāṃśāni dantyā bhāga-trayaṃ tathā ।
trivṛd-viśāle dvi-guṇe sātalā ca catur-guṇā ।।

eṣa nārāyaṇo nāma cūrṇo roga-gaṇāpahaḥ ।
nainaṃ prāpyābhivardhante rogā viṣṇum ivāsurāḥ ।।

ainaṃ prāpyātivartante
takreṇodaribhiḥ peyo gulmibhir badarāmbunā ।
ānāha-vāte surayā vāta-roge prasannayā ।।

dadhi-maṇḍena viṭ-saṅge dāḍimāmbhobhir arśasaiḥ ।
parikarte sa-vṛkṣāmlair uṣṇāmbubhir a-jīrṇake ।।

bhagandare pāṇḍu-roge kāse śvāse gala-grahe ।
hṛd-roge grahaṇī-doṣe kuṣṭhe mande anale jvare ।।

daṃṣṭrā-viṣe mūla-viṣe sa-gare kṛtrime doṣe ।
yathārhaṃ snigdha-koṣṭhena peyam etad virecanam ।।

hapuṣāṃ kāñcanakṣīrīṃ tri-phalāṃ nīlinī-phalam ।
trāyantīṃ rohiṇīṃ tiktāṃ sātalāṃ trivṛtāṃ vacām ।।

saindhavaṃ kāla-lavaṇaṃ pippalīṃ ceti cūrṇayet ।
dāḍima-tri-phalā-māṃsa-rasa-mūtra-sukhodakaiḥ ।।

peyo ayaṃ sarva-gulmeṣu plīhni sarvodareṣu ca ।
śvitre kuṣṭheṣv a-jarake sadane viṣame anale ।।

śophārśaḥ-pāṇḍu-rogeṣu kāmalāyāṃ halīmake ।
vāta-pitta-kaphāṃś cāśu virekeṇa prasādhayet ।।

nīlinīṃ niculaṃ vyoṣaṃ kṣārau lavaṇa-pañcakam ।
citrakaṃ ca pibec cūrṇaṃ sarpiṣodara-gulma-nut ।।

pūrva-vac ca pibed dugdhaṃ kṣāmaḥ śuddho antarāntarā ।
kārabhaṃ gavyam ājaṃ vā dadyād ātyayike gade ।।

snehān eva virekārthe dur-balebhyo viśeṣataḥ ।
harītakī-sūkṣma-rajaḥ-prastha-yuktaṃ ghṛtāḍhakam ।।

neham eva virekārthe
agnau vilāpya mathitaṃ khajena yava-pallake ।
nidhāpayet tato māsād uddhṛtaṃ gālitaṃ pacet ।।

harītakīnāṃ kvāthena dadhnā cāmlena saṃyutam ।
udaraṃ garaṃ aṣṭhīlām ānāhaṃ gulma-vidradhī ।।

hanty etat kuṣṭham unmādam apasmāraṃ ca pānataḥ ।
snuk-kṣīra-yuktād go-kṣīrāc chṛta-śītāt khajāhatāt ।।

yaj jātam ājyaṃ snuk-kṣīra-siddhaṃ tac ca tathā-guṇam ।
kṣīra-droṇaṃ sudhā-kṣīra-prasthārdha-sahitaṃ dadhi ।।

-prasthārdhena yutaṃ dadhi
jātaṃ mathitvā tat-sarpis trivṛt-siddhaṃ ca tad-guṇam ।
tathā siddhaṃ ghṛta-prasthaṃ payasy aṣṭa-guṇe pibet ।।

ayasy aṣṭa-guṇe pacet
snuk-kṣīra-pala-kalkena trivṛtā-ṣaṭ-palena ca ।
eṣāṃ cānu pibet peyāṃ rasaṃ svādu payo atha-vā ।।

ghṛte jīrṇe viriktaś ca koṣṇaṃ nāgara-sādhitam ।
pibed ambu tataḥ peyāṃ tato yūṣaṃ kulattha-jam ।।

pibed rūkṣas try-ahaṃ tv evaṃ bhūyo vā pratibhojitaḥ ।
punaḥ punaḥ pibet sarpir ānupūrvyānayaiva ca ।।

ghṛtāny etāni siddhāni vidadhyāt kuśalo bhiṣak ।
gulmānāṃ gara-doṣāṇām udarāṇāṃ ca śāntaye ।।

pīlu-kalkopasiddhaṃ vā ghṛtam ānāha-bhedanam ।
tailvakaṃ nīlinī-sarpiḥ snehaṃ vā miśrakaṃ pibet ।।

hṛta-doṣaḥ kramād aśnan laghu-śāly-odana-prati ।
upayuñjīta jaṭharī doṣa-śoṣa-nivṛttaye ।।

harītakī-sahasraṃ vā go-mūtreṇa payo-'nupaḥ ।
sahasraṃ pippalīnāṃ vā snuk-kṣīreṇa su-bhāvitam ।।

pippalī-vardhamānaṃ vā kṣīrāśī vā śilā-jatu ।
tad-vad vā gugguluṃ kṣīraṃ tulyārdraka-rasaṃ tathā ।।

ippalīṃ vardhamānaṃ vā
citrakāmaradārubhyāṃ kalkaṃ kṣīreṇa vā pibet ।
māsaṃ yuktas tathā hasti-pippalī-viśva-bheṣajam ।।

viḍaṅgaṃ citrako dantī cavyaṃ vyoṣaṃ ca taiḥ payaḥ ।
kalkaiḥ kola-samaiḥ pītvā pravṛddham udaraṃ jayet ।।

bhojyaṃ bhuñjīta vā māsaṃ snuhī-kṣīra-ghṛtānvitam ।
utkārikāṃ vā snuk-kṣīra-pīta-pathyā-kaṇā-kṛtām ।।

pārśva-śūlam upastambhaṃ hṛd-grahaṃ ca samīraṇaḥ ।
yadi kuryāt tatas tailaṃ bilva-kṣārānvitam pibet ।।

pakvaṃ vā ṭuṇṭuka-balā-palāśa-tila-nāla-jaiḥ ।
kṣāraiḥ kadaly-apāmārga-tarkārī-jaiḥ prṭhak-kṛtaiḥ ।।

kaphe vātena pitte vā tābhyāṃ vāpy āvṛte anile ।
balinaḥ svauṣadha-yutaṃ tailam eraṇḍa-jaṃ hitam ।।

devadāru-palāśārka-hasti-pippali-śigrukaiḥ ।
sāśvakarṇaiḥ sa-go-mūtraiḥ pradihyād udaraṃ bahiḥ ।।

vṛścikālī-vacā-śuṇṭhī-pañca-mūla-punarnavāt ।
varṣābhū-dhānya-kuṣṭhāc ca kvāthair mūtraiś ca secayet ।।

virikta-mlānam udaraṃ sveditaṃ śālvaṇādibhiḥ ।
vāsasā veṣṭayed evaṃ vāyur nādhmāpayet punaḥ ।।

veditaṃ śālvalādibhiḥ
su-viriktasya yasya syād ādhmānaṃ punar eva tam ।
su-snigdhair amla-lavaṇair nirūhaiḥ samupācaret ।।

sopastambho api vā vāyur ādhmāpayati yaṃ naram ।
tīkṣṇāḥ sa-kṣāra-go-mūtrāḥ śasyante tasya vastayaḥ ।।

iti sāmānyataḥ proktāḥ siddhā jaṭhariṇāṃ kriyāḥ ।
vātodare atha balinaṃ vidāry-ādi-śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।।

ti sāmānyataḥ proktā iddhā jaṭhariṇāṃ kriyā
pāyayeta tataḥ snigdhaṃ sveditāṅgaṃ virecayet ।
bahu-śas tailvakenainaṃ sarpiṣā miśrakeṇa vā ।।

kṛte saṃsarjane kṣīraṃ balārtham avacārayet ।
prāg utkleśān nivartyaṃ ca bale labdhe kramāt payaḥ ।।

rāg utkleśān nivarteta
yūṣai rasair vā mandāmla-lavaṇair edhitānalam ।
sodāvartaṃ punaḥ snigdha-svinnam āsthāpayet tataḥ ।।

tīkṣṇādho-bhāga-yuktena daśa-mūlika-vastinā ।
tilorubūka-tailena vāta-ghnāmla-śṛtena ca ।।

aśa-mūlena vastinā
sphuraṇākṣepa-saṃdhy-asthi-pārśva-pṛṣṭha-trikārtiṣu ।
rūkṣaṃ baddha-śakṛd-vātaṃ dīptāgnim anuvāsayet ।।

a-virecyasya śamanā vasti-kṣīra-ghṛtādayaḥ ।
balinaṃ svādu-siddhena paitte saṃsnehya sarpiṣā ।।

śyāmā-tribhaṇḍī-tri-phalā-vipakvena virecayet ।
sitā-madhu-ghṛtāḍhyena nirūho asya tato hitaḥ ।।

nyagrodhādi-kaṣāyeṇa sneha-vastiś ca tac-chṛtaḥ ।
dur-balaṃ tv anuvāsyādau śodhayet kṣīra-vastibhiḥ ।।

jāte cāgni-bale snigdhaṃ bhūyo bhūyo virecayet ।
kṣīreṇa sa-trivṛt-kalkenorubūka-śṛtena vā ।।

āte tv agni-bale snigdhaṃ ṃnorubūka-śṛtena tam
sātalā-trāyamāṇābhyāṃ śṛtenāragvadhena vā ।
sa-kaphe vā sa-mūtreṇa sa-tiktājyena sānile ।।

aptalā-trāyamāṇābhyāṃ
payasānya-tamenaiṣāṃ vidāry-ādi-śṛtena vā ।
bhuñjīta jaṭharaṃ cāsya pāyasenopanāhayet ।।

punaḥ kṣīraṃ punar vastiṃ punar eva virecanam ।
krameṇa dhruvam ātiṣṭhan yattaḥ pittodaraṃ jayet ।।

ataḥ pittodaraṃ jayet
vatsakādi-vipakvena kaphe saṃsnehya sarpiṣā ।
svinnaṃ snuk-kṣīra-siddhena bala-vantaṃ virecitam ।।

saṃsarjayet kaṭu-kṣāra-yuktair annaiḥ kaphāpahaiḥ ।
mūtra-try-ūṣaṇa-tailāḍhyo nirūho asya tato hitaḥ ।।

muṣkakādi-kaṣāyeṇa sneha-vastiś ca tac-chṛtaḥ ।
bhojanaṃ vyoṣa-dugdhena kaulatthena rasena vā ।।

staimityā-ruci-hṛl-lāse mande agnau madya-pāya ca ।
dadyād ariṣṭān kṣārāṃś ca kapha-styāna-sthirodare ।।

taimityā-ruci-hṛl-lāsair aphe styāne sthirodare
hiṅgūpakulye tri-phalāṃ devadāru niśā-dvayam ।
bhallātakaṃ śigru-phalaṃ kaṭukāṃ tiktakaṃ vacāṃ ।।

śuṇṭhīṃ mādrīṃ ghanaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ saralaṃ paṭu-pañcakam ।
dāhayej jarjarī-kṛtya dadhi-sneha-catuṣka-vat ।।

antar-dhūmaṃ tataḥ kṣārād biḍāla-padakaṃ pibet ।
madirā-dadhi-maṇḍoṣṇa-jalāriṣṭa-surāsavaiḥ ।।

-jalāriṣṭa-sudhāsavaiḥ
udaraṃ gulmam aṣṭhīlāṃ tūṇyau śophaṃ viṣūcikām ।
plīha-hṛd-roga-guda-jān udāvartaṃ ca nāśayet ।।

jayed ariṣṭa-go-mūtra-cūrṇāyas-kṛti-pānataḥ ।
sa-kṣāra-taila-pānaiś ca dur-balasya kaphodaram ।।

upanāhyaṃ sa-siddhārtha-kiṇvair bījaiś ca mūlakāt ।
kalkitair udaraṃ svedam abhīkṣṇaṃ cātra yojayet ।।

alkitair udara-svedam
saṃnipātodare kuryān nāti-kṣīṇa-balānale ।
doṣodrekānurodhena pratyākhyāya kriyām imām ।।

dantī-dravantī-phala-jaṃ tailaṃ pāne ca śasyate ।
kriyā-nivṛtte jaṭhare tri-doṣe tu viśeṣataḥ ।।

dadyād āpṛcchya taj-jñātīn pātuṃ madyena kalkitam ।
mūlaṃ kākādanī-guñjā-karavīraka-saṃbhavam ।।

pāna-bhojana-saṃyuktaṃ dadyād vā sthāvaraṃ viṣam ।
yasmin vā kupitaḥ sarpo vimuñcati phale viṣam ।।

tenāsya doṣa-saṃghātaḥ sthiro līno vi-mārga-gaḥ ।
bahiḥ pravartate bhinno viṣeṇāśu pramāthinā ।।

tathā vrajaty a-gada-tāṃ śarīrāntaram eva vā ।
hṛta-doṣaṃ tu śītāmbu-snātaṃ taṃ pāyayet payaḥ ।।

peyāṃ vā trivṛtaḥ śākaṃ māṇḍūkyā vāstukasya vā ।
kāla-śākaṃ yavākhyaṃ vā khādet sva-rasa-sādhitam ।।

nir-amla-lavaṇa-snehaṃ svinnā-svinnam an-anna-bhuk ।
māsam ekaṃ tataś caiva tṛṣitaḥ sva-rasaṃ pibet ।।

āsam ekaṃ tataś caivaṃ
evaṃ vinirhṛte śākair doṣe māsāt paraṃ tataḥ ।
dur-balāya prayuñjīta prāṇa-bhṛt kārabhaṃ payaḥ ।।

plīhodare yathā-doṣaṃ snigdhasya sveditasya ca ।
sirāṃ bhukta-vato dadhnā vāma-bāhau vimokṣayet ।।

labdhe bale ca bhūyo api sneha-pītaṃ viśodhitam ।
samudra-śukti-jaṃ kṣāraṃ payasā pāyayet tathā ।।

amla-srutaṃ viḍa-kaṇā-cūrṇāḍhyaṃ naktamāla-jam ।
śaubhāñjanasya vā kvāthaṃ saindhavāgni-kaṇānvitam ।।

hiṅgv-ādi-cūrṇaṃ kṣārājyaṃ yuñjīta ca yathā-balam ।
pippalī-nāgaraṃ dantī-samāṃśaṃ dvi-guṇābhayam ।।

-samāṃśaṃ dvi-guṇābhayā
viḍārdhāṃśa-yutaṃ cūrṇam idam uṣṇāmbunā pibet ।
viḍaṅgaṃ citrakaṃ saktūn sa-ghṛtān saindhavaṃ vacām ।।

dagdhvā kapāle payasā gulma-plīhāpahaṃ pibet ।
tailonmiśrair badaraka-pattraiḥ saṃmarditaiḥ samupanaddhaḥ ।।

musalena pīḍito anu ca yāti plīhā payo-bhujo nāśam ।
rohītaka-latāḥ kḷptāḥ khaṇḍa-śaḥ sābhayā jale ।।

mūtre vāsunuyāt tac ca sapta-rātra-sthitaṃ pibet ।
kāmalā-plīha-gulmārśaḥ-kṛmi-mehodarāpaham ।।

ūtre vāsunuyāt tat tu
rohītaka-tvacaḥ kṛtvā palānāṃ pañca-viṃśatim ।
kola-dvi-prastha-saṃyuktaṃ kaṣāyam upakalpayet ।।

pālikaiḥ pañca-kolais tu taiḥ samastaiś ca tulyayā ।
rohītaka-tvacā piṣṭair ghṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।।

plīhābhivṛddhiṃ śamayaty etad āśu prayojitam ।
kadalyās tila-nālānāṃ kṣāreṇa kṣurakasya ca ।।

līhābhivṛddhiṃ śamayed c plīhāti-vṛddhiṃ śamayaty 
kṣāreṇekṣurakasya ca
tailaṃ pakvaṃ jayet pānāt plīhānaṃ kapha-vāta-jam ।
a-śāntau gulma-vidhinā yojayed agni-karma ca ।।

a-prāpta-picchā-salile plīhni vāta-kapholbaṇe ।
paittike jīvanīyāni sarpīṃṣi kṣīra-vastayaḥ ।।

raktāvasekaḥ saṃśuddhiḥ kṣīra-pānaṃ ca śasyate ।
yakṛti plīha-vat karma dakṣiṇe tu bhuje sirām ।।

svinnāya baddhodariṇe mūtra-tīkṣṇauṣadhānvitam ।
sa-taila-lavaṇaṃ dadyān nirūhaṃ sānuvāsanam ।।

parisraṃsīni cānnāni tīkṣṇaṃ cāsmai virecanam ।
udāvarta-haraṃ karma kāryaṃ yac cānilāpaham ।।

chidrodaram ṛte svedāc chleṣmodara-vad ācaret ।
jātaṃ jātaṃ jalaṃ srāvyam evaṃ tad yāpayed bhiṣak ।।

apāṃ doṣa-harāṇy ādau yojayed udakodare ।
mūtra-yuktāni tīkṣṇāni vividha-kṣāra-vanti ca ।।

dīpanīyaiḥ kapha-ghnaiś ca tam āhārair upācaret ।
kṣāraṃ chāga-karīṣāṇāṃ srutaṃ mūtre agninā pacet ।।

ghanī-bhavati tasmiṃś ca karṣāṃśaṃ cūrṇitaṃ kṣipet ।
pippalī pippalī-mūlaṃ śuṇṭhī lavaṇa-pañcakam ।।

nikumbha-kumbha-tri-phalā-svarṇakṣīrī-viṣāṇikāḥ ।
svarjikā-kṣāra-ṣaḍgranthā-sātalā-yava-śūka-jam ।।

kolābhā guṭikāḥ kṛtvā tataḥ sauvīrakāplutāḥ ।
pibed a-jarake śophe pravṛddhe codakodare ।।

ravṛddhe ca dakodare
ity auṣadhair a-praśame triṣu baddhodarādiṣu ।
prayuñjīta bhiṣak śastram ārta-bandhu-nṛpārthitaḥ ।।

snigdha-svinna-tanor nābher adho baddha-kṣatāntrayoḥ ।
pāṭayed udaraṃ muktvā vāmataś catur-aṅgulāt ।।

catur-aṅgula-mānaṃ tu niṣkāsyāntrāṇi tena ca ।
nirīkṣyāpanayed vāla-mala-lepopalādikam ।।

chidre tu śalyam uddhṛtya viśodhyāntra-parisravam ।
markoṭair daṃśayec chidraṃ teṣu lagneṣu cāharet ।।

iśodhyāntraṃ parisravam
kāyaṃ mūrdhno anu cāntrāṇi yathā-sthānaṃ niveśayet ।
aktāni madhu-sarpirbhyām atha sīvyed bahir vraṇam ।।

athā-sthānaṃ viveśayet
tataḥ kṛṣṇa-mṛdālipya badhnīyād yaṣṭi-miśrayā ।
nivāta-sthaḥ payo-vṛttiḥ sneha-droṇyāṃ vaset tataḥ ।।

sa-jale jaṭhare tailair abhyaktasyānilāpahaiḥ ।
svinnasyoṣṇāmbunā-kakṣam udare paṭṭa-veṣṭite ।।

dare pariveṣṭite
baddha-cchidrodita-sthāne vidhyed aṅgula-mātrakam ।
nidhāya tasmin nāḍīṃ ca srāvayed ardham ambhasaḥ ।।

athāsya nāḍīm ākṛṣya tailena lavaṇena ca ।
vraṇam abhyajya baddhvā ca veṣṭayed vāsasodaram ।।

tṛtīye ahni caturthe vā yāvad ā-ṣo-ḍaśaṃ dinam ।
tasya viśramya viśramya srāvayed alpa-śo jalam ।।

āvad vā-dina-ṣo-ḍaśa
viveṣṭayed gāḍha-taraṃ jaṭharaṃ vāsasā ślatham ।
niḥsrute laṅghitaḥ peyām a-sneha-lavaṇāṃ pibet ।।

aṭharaṃ ca ślathā-ślatham
syāt kṣīra-vṛttiḥ ṣaṇ-māsāṃś trīn peyāṃ payasā pibet ।
trīṃś cānyān payasaivādyāt phalāmlena rasena vā ।।

alpa-śo a-sneha-lavaṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ śyāmāka-kodravam ।
prayato vatsareṇaivaṃ vijayeta jalodaram ।।

varjyeṣu yantrito diṣṭe nāty-a-diṣṭe jitendriyaḥ ।
sarvam evodaraṃ prāyo doṣa-saṃghāta-jaṃ yataḥ ।।

ato vātādi-śamanī kriyā sarva-tra śasyate ।
vahnir manda-tvam āyāti doṣaiḥ kukṣau prapūrite ।।

riyā sarvā praśasyate
tasmād bhojyāni bhojyāni dīpanāni laghūni ca ।
sa-pañca-mūlāny alpāmla-paṭu-sneha-kaṭūni ca ।।

bhāvitānāṃ gavāṃ mūtre ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca taṇḍulaiḥ ।
yavāgūṃ payasā siddhāṃ pra-kāmaṃ bhojayen naram ।।

pibed ikṣu-rasaṃ cānu jaṭharāṇāṃ nivṛttaye ।
svaṃ svaṃ sthānaṃ vrajanty eṣāṃ vāta-pitta-kaphās tathā ।।

aty-arthoṣṇāmla-lavaṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ grāhi himaṃ guru ।
guḍaṃ taila-kṛtaṃ śākaṃ vāri pānāvagāhayoḥ ।।

ty-arthoṣṇāmbu-lavaṇaṃ
āyāsādhva-divā-svapna-yānāni ca parityajet ।
nāty-accha-sāndra-madhuraṃ takraṃ pāne praśasyate ।।

sa-kaṇā-lavaṇaṃ vāte pitte soṣaṇa-śarkaram ।
yavānī-saindhavājājī-madhu-vyoṣaiḥ kaphodare ।।

try-ūṣaṇa-kṣāra-lavaṇaiḥ saṃyutaṃ nicayodare ।
madhu-taila-vacā-śuṇṭhī-śatāhvā-kuṣṭha-saindhavaiḥ ।।

adhu-taila-varā-śuṇṭhī- adhu-taila-vasā-śuṇṭhī-
plīhni baddhe tu hapuṣā-yavānī-paṭv-ajājibhiḥ ।
sa-kṛṣṇā-mākṣikaṃ chidre vyoṣa-vat salilodare ।।

gauravā-rocakānāha-manda-vahny-atisāriṇām ।
takraṃ vāta-kaphārtānām amṛta-tvāya kalpate ।।

prayogāṇāṃ ca sarveṣām anu kṣīraṃ prayojayet ।
sthairya-kṛt sarva-dhātūnāṃ balyaṃ doṣānubandha-hṛt ।।
bheṣajāpacitāṅgānāṃ kṣīram evāmṛtāyate ।।
cikitsāsthāna
pāṇḍv-āmayī pibet sarpir ādau kalyāṇakāhvayam ।
pañca-gavyaṃ mahā-tiktaṃ śṛtaṃ vāragvadhādinā ।।

āṇḍu-rogī pibet sarpir
dāḍimāt kuḍavo dhānyāt kuḍavārdhaṃ palaṃ palam ।
citrakāc chṛṅgaverāc ca pippaly-ardha-palaṃ ca taiḥ ।।

kalkitair viṃśati-palaṃ ghṛtasya salilāḍhake ।
siddhaṃ hṛt-pāṇḍu-gulmārśaḥ-plīha-vāta-kaphārti-nut ।।

dīpanaṃ śvāsa-kāsa-ghnaṃ mūḍha-vātānulomanam ।
duḥkha-prasavinīnāṃ ca vandhyānāṃ ca praśasyate ।।

snehitaṃ vāmayet tīkṣṇaiḥ punaḥ snigdhaṃ ca śodhayet ।
payasā mūtra-yuktena bahu-śaḥ kevalena vā ।।

dantī-phala-rase koṣṇe kāśmaryāñjalim āsutam ।
drākṣāñjaliṃ vā mṛditaṃ tat pibet pāṇḍu-roga-jit ।।

antī-pala-rase koṣṇe
mūtreṇa piṣṭāṃ pathyāṃ vā tat-siddhaṃ vā phala-trayam ।
svarṇakṣīrī-trivṛc-chyāmā-bhadradāru-mahauṣadham ।।

go-mūtrāñjalinā piṣṭaṃ śṛtaṃ tenaiva vā pibet ।
sādhitaṃ kṣīram ebhir vā pibed doṣānulomanam ।।

mūtre sthitaṃ vā saptāhaṃ payasāyo-rajaḥ pibet ।
jīrṇe kṣīreṇa bhuñjīta rasena madhureṇa vā ।।

śuddhaś cobhayato lihyāt pathyāṃ madhu-ghṛta-drutām ।
viśālā-kaṭukā-mustā-kuṣṭha-dāru-kaliṅgakāḥ ।।

athyā madhu-ghṛta-drutāḥ iśālāṃ kaṭukāṃ mustāṃ 
kuṣṭhaṃ dāru-kaliṅgakāḥ
karṣāṃśā dvi-picur mūrvā karṣārdhāṃśā ghuṇapriyā ।
pītvā tac cūrṇam ambhobhiḥ sukhair lihyāt tato madhu ।।

pāṇḍu-rogaṃ jvaraṃ dāhaṃ kāsaṃ śvāsam a-rocakam ।
gulmānāhāma-vātāṃś ca rakta-pittaṃ ca taj jayet ।।

vāsā-guḍūcī-tri-phalā-kaṭvī-bhūnimba-nimba-jaḥ ।
kvāthaḥ kṣaudra-yuto hanti pāṇḍu-pittāsra-kāmalāḥ ।।

vyoṣāgni-vella-tri-phalā-mustais tulyam ayo-rajaḥ ।
cūrṇitaṃ takra-madhv-ājya-koṣṇāmbhobhiḥ prayojitam ।।

kāmalā-pāṇḍu-hṛd-roga-kuṣṭhārśo-meha-nāśanam ।
guḍa-nāgara-maṇḍūra-tilāṃśān mānataḥ samān ।।

pippalī-dvi-guṇān dadyād guṭikāṃ pāṇḍu-rogiṇe ।
tāpyaṃ dārvyās tvacaṃ cavyaṃ granthikaṃ devadāru ca ।।

vyoṣādi-navakaṃ caitac cūrṇayed dvi-guṇaṃ tataḥ ।
maṇḍūraṃ cāñjana-nibhaṃ sarvato aṣṭa-guṇe atha tat ।।

yoṣādi-navakaṃ ceti
pṛthag vipakve go-mūtre vaṭakī-karaṇa-kṣame ।
prakṣipya vaṭakān kuryāt tān khādet takra-bhojanaḥ ।।

ete maṇḍūra-vaṭakāḥ prāṇa-dāḥ pāṇḍu-rogiṇām ।
kuṣṭhāny a-jarakaṃ śopham ūru-stambham a-rocakam ।।

arśāṃsi kāmalāṃ mehān plīhānaṃ śamayanti ca ।
tāpyādri-jatu-raupyāyo-malāḥ pañca-palāḥ pṛthak ।।

citraka-tri-phalā-vyoṣa-viḍaṅgaiḥ pālikaiḥ saha ।
śarkarāṣṭa-palonmiśrāś cūrṇitā madhunā drutāḥ ।।

ūrṇitā madhunā yutāḥ ūrṇitāḥ sa-madhu-drutāḥ
pāṇḍu-rogaṃ viṣaṃ kāsaṃ yakṣmāṇaṃ viṣamaṃ jvaram ।
kuṣṭhāny a-jarakaṃ mehaṃ śophaṃ śvāsam a-rocakam ।।

viśeṣād dhanty apasmāraṃ kāmalāṃ guda-jāni ca ।
kauṭaja-tri-phalā-nimba-paṭola-ghana-nāgaraiḥ ।।

bhāvitāni daśāhāni rasair dvi-tri-guṇāni vā ।
śilā-jatu-palāny aṣṭau tāvatī sita-śarkarā ।।

tvakkṣīrī-pippalī-dhātrī-karkaṭākhyāḥ palonmitāḥ ।
nidigdhyāḥ phala-mūlābhyāṃ palaṃ yuktyā tri-jātakam ।।

idigdhā-phala-mūlābhyāṃ
madhu-tri-pala-saṃyuktān kuryād akṣa-samān guḍān ।
dāḍimāmbu-payaḥ-pakṣi-rasa-toya-surāsavān ।।

adhu-tri-pala-saṃyuktaṃ
tān bhakṣayitvānupiben nir-anno bhukta eva vā ।
pāṇḍu-kuṣṭha-jvara-plīha-tamakārśo-bhagandaram ।।

hṛn-mūtra-pūti-śukrāgni-doṣa-śoṣa-garodaram ।
kāsāsṛg-dara-pittāsṛk-śopha-gulma-galāmayān ।।

meha-vardhma-bhramān hanyuḥ sarva-doṣa-harāḥ śivāḥ ।
drākṣā-prasthaṃ kaṇā-prasthaṃ śarkarārdha-tulāṃ tathā ।।

dvi-palaṃ madhukaṃ śuṇṭhīṃ tvakkṣīrīṃ ca vicūrṇitam ।
dhātrī-phala-rasa-droṇe tat kṣiptvā leha-vat pacet ।।

śītān madhu-prastha-yutād lihyāt pāṇi-talaṃ tataḥ ।
halīmakaṃ pāṇḍu-rogaṃ kāmalāṃ ca niyacchati ।।

kanīyaḥ-pañca-mūlāmbu śasyate pāna-bhojane ।
pāṇḍūnāṃ kāmalārtānāṃ mṛdvīkāmalakād rasaḥ ।।

iti sāmānyataḥ proktaṃ pāṇḍu-roge bhiṣag-jitam ।
vikalpya yojyaṃ viduṣā pṛthag doṣa-balaṃ prati ।।

āṇḍu-roga-bhiṣag-jitam
sneha-prāyaṃ pavana-je tikta-śītaṃ tu paittike ।
ślaiṣmike kaṭu-rūkṣoṣṇaṃ vimiśraṃ sāṃnipātike ।।

ślaiṣmike kaṭu-tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ imiśraṃ saṃnipāta-je
mṛdaṃ niryāpayet kāyāt tīkṣṇaiḥ saṃśodhanaiḥ puraḥ ।
balādhānāni sarpīṃṣi śuddhe koṣṭhe tu yojayet ।।

ṛdaṃ nirvāpayet kāyāt śuddhe koṣṭhe niyojayet
vyoṣa-bilva-dvi-rajanī-tri-phalā-dvi-punarnavam ।
mustāny ayo-rajaḥ pāṭhā viḍaṅgaṃ devadāru ca ।।

vṛścikālī ca bhārgī ca sa-kṣīrais taiḥ śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।
sarvān praśamayaty āśu vikārān mṛttikā-kṛtān ।।

tad-vat kesara-yaṣṭy-āhva-pippalī-kṣīra-śādvalaiḥ ।
mṛd-dveṣaṇāya tal-laulye vitared bhāvitāṃ mṛdam ।।

vellāgni-nimba-prasavaiḥ pāṭhayā mūrvayātha-vā ।
mṛd-bheda-bhinna-doṣānugamād yojyaṃ ca bheṣajam ।।

kāmalāyāṃ tu pitta-ghnaṃ pāṇḍu-rogā-virodhi yat ।
pathyā-śata-rase pathyā-vṛntārdha-śata-kalkitaḥ ।।

prasthaḥ siddho ghṛtād gulma-kāmalā-pāṇḍu-roga-nut ।
āragvadhaṃ rasenekṣor vidāry-āmalakasya vā ।।

sa-try-ūṣaṇaṃ bilva-mātraṃ pāyayet kāmalāpaham ।
piben nikumbha-kalkaṃ vā dvi-guḍaṃ śīta-vāriṇā ।।

vi-guṇaṃ śīta-vāriṇā
kumbhasya cūrṇaṃ sa-kṣaudraṃ traiphalena rasena vā ।
tri-phalāyā guḍūcyā vā dārvyā nimbasya vā rasam ।।

prātaḥ prātar madhu-yutaṃ kāmalārtāya yojayet ।
niśā-gairika-dhātrībhiḥ kāmalāpaham añjanam ।।

śilā-gairika-dhātrībhiḥ
tila-piṣṭa-nibhaṃ yas tu kāmalā-vān sṛjen malam ।
kapha-ruddha-pathaṃ tasya pittaṃ kapha-harair jayet ।।

rūkṣa-śīta-guru-svādu-vyāyāma-bala-nigrahaiḥ ।
kapha-saṃmūrchito vāyur yadā pittaṃ bahiḥ kṣipet ।।

hāridra-netra-mūtra-tvak śveta-varcās tadā naraḥ ।
bhavet sāṭopa-viṣṭambho guruṇā hṛdayena ca ।।

daurbalyālpāgni-pārśvārti-hidhmā-śvāsā-ruci-jvaraiḥ ।
krameṇālpe anuṣajyeta pitte śākhā-samāśrite ।।

rasais taṃ rūkṣa-kaṭv-amlaiḥ śikhi-tittiri-dakṣa-jaiḥ ।
śuṣka-mūlaka-jair yūṣaiḥ kulatthotthaiś ca bhojayet ।।

bhṛśāmla-tīkṣṇa-kaṭuka-lavaṇoṣṇaṃ ca śasyate ।
sa-bījapūraka-rasaṃ lihyād vyoṣaṃ tathāśayam ।।

svaṃ pittam eti tenāsya śakṛd apy anurajyate ।
vāyuś ca yāti praśamaṃ sahāṭopādy-upadravaiḥ ।।

nivṛttopadravasyāsya kāryaḥ kāmaliko vidhiḥ ।
go-mūtreṇa pibet kumbha-kāmalāyāṃ śilā-jatu ।।

māsaṃ mākṣika-dhātuṃ vā kiṭṭaṃ vātha hiraṇya-jam ।
guḍūcī-sva-rasa-kṣīra-sādhitena halīmakī ।।

mahiṣī-haviṣā snigdhaḥ pibed dhātrī-rasena tu ।
trivṛtāṃ tad-virikto adyāt svādu pittānilāpaham ।।

drākṣā-lehaṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ sarpīṃṣi madhurāṇi ca ।
yāpanān kṣīra-vastīṃś ca śīlayet sānuvāsanān ।।

mārdvīkāriṣṭa-yogāṃś ca pibed yuktyāgni-vṛddhaye ।
kāsikaṃ cābhayā-lehaṃ pippalīṃ madhukaṃ balām ।।

āsikaṃ vābhayā-lehaṃ
payasā ca prayuñjīta yathā-doṣaṃ yathā-balam ।
pāṇḍu-rogeṣu kuśalaḥ śophoktaṃ ca kriyā-kramam ।।

ayas-tila-try-ūṣaṇa-kola-bhāgaiḥ sarvaiḥ samaṃ mākṣika-dhātu-cūrṇam ।
tair modakaḥ kṣaudra-yuto anu-takraḥ pāṇḍv-āmaye dūra-gate api śastaḥ ।।

cikitsāsthāna
sarva-tra sarvāṅga-sare doṣa-je śvayathau purā ।
sāme viśoṣito bhuktvā laghu koṣṇāmbhasā pibet ।।

nāgarātiviṣā-dāru-viḍaṅgendrayavoṣaṇam ।
atha-vā vijayā-śuṇṭhī-devadāru-punarnavam ।।

navāyasaṃ vā doṣāḍhyaḥ śuddhyai mūtra-harītakīḥ ।
varā-kvāthena kaṭukā-kumbhāyas-try-ūṣaṇāni ca ।।

śuddhyai mūtra-harītakīm
atha-vā gugguluṃ tad-vaj jatu vā śaila-saṃbhavam ।
mandāgniḥ śīlayed āma-guru-bhinna-vibandha-viṭ ।।

takraṃ sauvarcala-vyoṣa-kṣaudra-yuktaṃ guḍābhayām ।
takrānu-pānām atha-vā tad-vad vā guḍa-nāgaram ।।

ārdrakaṃ vā sama-guḍaṃ prakuñcārdha-vivardhitam ।
paraṃ pañca-palaṃ māsaṃ yūṣa-kṣīra-rasāśanaḥ ।।

gulmodarārśaḥ-śvayathu-pramehāñ chvāsa-pratiśyālasakā-vipākān ।
sa-kāmalā-śoṣa-mano-vikārān kāsaṃ kaphaṃ caiva jayet prayogaḥ ।।

ghṛtam ārdraka-nāgarasya kalka-sva-rasābhyāṃ payasā ca sādhayitvā ।
śvayathu-kṣavathūdarāgni-sādair abhibhūto api piban bhavaty a-rogaḥ ।।

rasas tathaivārdraka-nāgarasya peyo atha jīrṇe payasānnam adyāt ।
śilāhvayaṃ vā tri-phalā-rasena hanyāt tri-doṣaṃ śvayathuṃ prasahya ।।

punarnavā-nimba-paṭola-śuṇṭhī- tiktāmṛtā-dārvy-abhayā-kaṣāyaḥ ।
sarvāṅga-śophodara-kāsa-śūla-śvāsānvitaṃ pāṇḍu-gadaṃ ca hanti ।।

nir-āmo baddha-śamalaḥ pibec chvayathu-pīḍitaḥ ।
tri-kaṭu-trivṛtā-dantī-citrakaiḥ sādhitaṃ payaḥ ।।

mūtraṃ gor vā mahiṣyā vā sa-kṣīraṃ kṣīra-bhojanaḥ ।
saptāhaṃ māsaṃ atha-vā syād uṣṭra-kṣīra-vartanaḥ ।।

yād uṣṭrī-kṣīra-vartanaḥ
yavānakaṃ yava-kṣāraṃ yavānīṃ pañca-kolakam ।
maricaṃ dāḍimaṃ pāṭhāṃ dhānakām amla-vetasam ।।

bāla-bilvaṃ ca karṣāṃśaṃ sādhayet salilāḍhake ।
tena pakvo ghṛta-prasthaḥ śophārśo-gulma-meha-hā ।।

dadhnaś citraka-garbhād vā ghṛtaṃ tat-takra-saṃyutam ।
pakvaṃ sa-citrakaṃ tad-vad guṇair yuñjyāc ca kāla-vit ।।

dhānvantaraṃ mahā-tiktaṃ kalyāṇam abhayā-ghṛtam ।
daśa-mūla-kaṣāyasya kaṃse pathyā-śataṃ pacet ।।

dattvā guḍa-tulāṃ tasmin lehe dadyād vicūrṇitam ।
tri-jātakaṃ tri-kaṭukaṃ kiñ-cic ca yava-śūka-jam ।।
prasthārdhaṃ ca hime kṣaudrāt tan nihanty upayojitam ।।pravṛddha-śopha-jvara-meha-gulma-kārśyāma-vātāmlaka-rakta-pittam ।।vaivarṇya-mūtrānila-śukra-doṣa-śvāsā-ruci-plīha-garodaraṃ ca ।।purāṇa-yava-śāly-annaṃ daśa-mūlāmbu-sādhitam ।।
alpam alpa-paṭu-snehaṃ bhojanaṃ śvayathor hitam ।
kṣāra-vyoṣānvitair maudgaiḥ kaulatthaiḥ sa-kaṇai rasaiḥ ।।

hojanaṃ śvayathau hitam
tathā jāṅgala-jaiḥ kūrma-godhā-śalyaka-jair api ।
an-amlaṃ mathitaṃ pāne madyāny auṣadha-vanti ca ।।

ajājī-śaṭhī-jivantī-kāravī-pauṣkarāgnikaiḥ ।
bilva-madhya-yava-kṣāra-vṛkṣāmlair badaronmitaiḥ ।।

kṛtā peyājya-tailābhyāṃ yukti-bhṛṣṭā paraṃ hitā ।
śophātīsāra-hṛd-roga-gulmārśo-'lpāgni-mehinām ।।

guṇais tad-vac ca pāṭhāyāḥ pañca-kolena sādhitā ।
śaileya-kuṣṭha-sthauṇeya-reṇukāguru-padmakaiḥ ।।

śrīveṣṭaka-nakha-spṛkkā-devadāru-priyaṅgubhiḥ ।
māṃsī-māgadhikā-vanya-dhānya-dhyāmaka-vālakaiḥ ।।

catur-jātaka-tālīśa-mustā-gandha-palāśakaiḥ ।
kuryād abhyañjanaṃ tailaṃ lepaṃ snānāya tūdakam ।।

snānaṃ vā nimba-varṣābhū-naktamālārka-vāriṇā ।
ekāṅga-śophe varṣābhū-karavīraka-kiṃśukaiḥ ।।

viśālā-tri-phalā-lodhra-nalikā-devadārubhiḥ ।
hiṃsrā-kośātakī-mādrī-tālaparṇī-jayantibhiḥ ।।

sthūla-kākādanī-śāla-nākulī-vṛṣaparṇibhiḥ ।
vṛddhyarddhi-hastikarṇaiś ca sukhoṣṇair lepanaṃ hitam ।।

athānilotthe śvayathau māsārdhaṃ trivṛtaṃ pibet ।
tailam eraṇḍa-jaṃ vāta-viḍ-vibandhe tad eva tu ।।

prāg-bhaktaṃ payasā yuktaṃ rasair vā kārayet tathā ।
svedābhyaṅgān samīra-ghnān lepam ekāṅga-ge punaḥ ।।

mātuluṅgāgnimanthena śuṇṭhī-hiṃsrāmarāhvayaiḥ ।
paitte tiktaṃ pibet sarpir nyagrodhādyena vā śṛtam ।।

kṣīraṃ tṛḍ-dāha-moheṣu lepābhyaṅgāś ca śītalāḥ ।
paṭola-mūla-trāyantī-yaṣṭy-āhva-kaṭukābhayāḥ ।।

aṭola-mūrvā-trāyantī-
dāru dārvī himaṃ dantī viśālā niculaṃ kaṇā ।
taiḥ kvāthaḥ sa-ghṛtaḥ pīto hanty antas-tāpa-tṛḍ-bhramān ।।

at-kvāthaḥ sa-ghṛtaḥ pīto
sa-saṃnipāta-vīsarpa-śopha-dāha-viṣa-jvarān ।
āragvadhādinā siddhaṃ tailaṃ śleṣmodbhave pibet ।।

-śopha-dāha-mada-jvarān
sroto-vibandhe mande agnāv a-rucau stimitāśayaḥ ।
kṣāra-cūrṇāsavāriṣṭa-mūtra-takrāṇi śīlayet ।।

kṛṣṇā-purāṇa-piṇyāka-śigru-tvak-sikatātasīḥ ।
praleponmardane yuñjyāt sukhoṣṇā mūtra-kalkitāḥ ।।

snānaṃ mūtrāmbhasī siddhe kuṣṭha-tarkāri-citrakaiḥ ।
kulattha-nāgarābhyāṃ vā caṇḍāguru vilepane ।।

kālājaśṛṅgī-sarala-bastagandhā-hayāhvayāḥ ।
ekaiṣīkā ca lepaḥ syāc chvayathāv eka-gātra-ge ।।

yaṣṭī-dugdha-tilair lepo nava-nītena saṃyutaḥ ।
śopham āruṣkaraṃ hanti vṛntaiḥ śāla-dalasya vā ।।

yathā-doṣaṃ yathāsannaṃ śuddhiṃ raktāvasecanam ।
kurvīta miśra-doṣe tu doṣodreka-balāt kriyām ।।

ajāji-pāṭhā-ghana-pañca-kola-vyāghrī-rajanyaḥ sukha-toya-pītāḥ ।
śophaṃ tri-doṣaṃ cira-jaṃ pravṛddhaṃ nighnanti bhūnimba-mahauṣadhe ca ।।

amṛtā-dvitayaṃ śivātikā surakāṣṭhaṃ sa-puraṃ sa-go-jalam ।
śvayathūdara-kuṣṭha-pāṇḍu-tā-kṛmi-mehordhva-kaphānilāpaham ।।

iti nijam adhikṛtya pathyam uktaṃ kṣata-janite kṣata-jaṃ viśodhanīyam ।
sruti-hima-ghṛta-lepa-seka-rekair viṣa-janite viṣa-jic ca śopha iṣṭam ।।
grāmyāb-jānūpaṃ piśitam a-balaṃ śuṣka-śākaṃ tilānnaṃ ।।gauḍaṃ piṣṭānnaṃ dadhi sa-lavaṇaṃ vijjalaṃ madyam amlam ।।
auḍaṃ piṣṭānnaṃ dadhi sa-lavaṇaṃ nir-jalaṃ madyam amlam dhānā vallūraṃ samaśanam atho gurv a-sātmyaṃ vidāhi ।।
svapnaṃ cā-rātrau śvayathu-gada-vān varjayen maithunaṃ ca ।।
cikitsāsthāna
ādāv eva visarpeṣu hitaṃ laṅghana-rūkṣaṇam ।
raktāvaseko vamanaṃ virekaḥ snehanaṃ na tu ।।

pracchardanaṃ visarpa-ghnaṃ sa-yaṣṭīndrayavaṃ phalam ।
paṭola-pippalī-nimba-pallavair vā samanvitam ।।

rasena yuktaṃ trāyantyā drākṣāyās traiphalena vā ।
virecanaṃ trivṛc-cūrṇaṃ payasā sarpiṣātha-vā ।।

yojyaṃ koṣṭha-gate doṣe viśeṣeṇa viśodhanam ।
a-viśodhyasya doṣe alpe śamanaṃ candanotpalam ।।

musta-nimba-paṭolaṃ vā paṭolādikam eva vā ।
śārivāmalakośīra-mustaṃ vā kvathitaṃ jale ।।

durālabhāṃ parpaṭakaṃ guḍūcīṃ viśva-bheṣajam ।
pākyaṃ śīta-kaṣāyaṃ vā tṛṣṇā-visarpa-vān pibet ।।

dārvī-paṭola-kaṭukā-masūra-tri-phalās tathā ।
sa-nimba-yaṣṭī-trāyantīḥ kvathitā ghṛta-mūrchitāḥ ।।
amṛta-vṛṣa-paṭolaṃ mustakaṃ saptaparṇaṃ ।।khadiram asita-vetraṃ nimba-pattraṃ haridre ।।vividha-viṣa-visarpān kuṣṭha-visphoṭa-kaṇḍūr ।।apanayati masūrīṃ śīta-pittaṃ jvaraṃ ca ।।
śākhā-duṣṭe tu rudhire raktam evādito haret ।
tvaṅ-māṃsa-snāyu-saṃkledo rakta-kledād dhi jāyate ।।

nir-āme śleṣmaṇi kṣīṇe vāta-pittottare hitam ।
ghṛtaṃ tiktaṃ mahā-tiktaṃ śṛtaṃ vā trāyamāṇayā ।।

nirhṛte asre viśuddhe antar-doṣe tvaṅ-māṃsa-saṃdhi-ge ।
bahiḥ-kriyāḥ pradehādyāḥ sadyo visarpa-śāntaye ।।

śatāhvā-musta-vārāhī-vaṃśārtagala-dhānyakam ।
surāhvā kṛṣṇagandhā ca kuṣṭhaṃ cālepanaṃ cale ।।

uṣṭhaṃ vālepanaṃ cale
nyagrodhādi-gaṇaḥ pitte tathā padmotpalādikam ।
nyagrodha-pādās taruṇāḥ kadalī-garbha-saṃyutāḥ ।।

bisa-granthiś ca lepaḥ syāc chata-dhauta-ghṛtāplutaḥ ।
padminī-kardamaḥ śītaḥ piṣṭaṃ mauktikam eva vā ।।

śaṅkhaḥ pravālaṃ śuktir vā gairikaṃ vā ghṛtānvitam ।
tri-phalā-padmakośīra-samaṅgā-karavīrakam ।।

-samaṅgā-karavīra-jam
nala-mūlāny anantā ca lepaḥ śleṣma-visarpa-hā ।
dhava-saptāhva-khadira-devadāru-kuraṇṭakam ।।

sa-mustāragvadhaṃ lepo vargo vā varuṇādikaḥ ।
āragvadhasya pattrāṇi tvacaḥ śleṣmātakodbhavāḥ ।।

indrāṇi-śākaṃ kākāhvā śirīṣa-kusumāni ca ।
seka-vraṇābhyaṅga-havir-lepa-cūrṇān yathā-yatham ।।

ndrāṇi-śāka-kākāhvā- -śirīṣa-kusumāni ca
etair evauṣadhaiḥ kuryād vāyau lepā ghṛtādhikāḥ ।
kapha-sthāna-gate sāme pitta-sthāna-gate atha-vā ।।

a-śītoṣṇā hitā rūkṣā rakta-pitte ghṛtānvitāḥ ।
aty-artha-śītās tanavas tanu-vastrāntarā-sthitāḥ ।।

anu-vastrāntara-sthitāḥ
yojyāḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe anye anye manda-vīryās ta eva ca ।
saṃsṛṣṭa-doṣe saṃsṛṣṭam etat karma praśasyate ।।

śata-dhauta-ghṛtenāgniṃ pradihyāt kevalena vā ।
secayed ghṛta-maṇḍena śītena madhukāmbunā ।।

sitāmbhasāmbho-da-jalaiḥ kṣīreṇekṣu-rasena vā ।
pāna-lepana-sekeṣu mahā-tiktaṃ paraṃ hitam ।।

itāmbhasāmbho-ja-jalaiḥ
granthy-ākhye rakta-pitta-ghnaṃ kṛtvā samyag yathoditam ।
kaphānila-ghnaṃ karmeṣṭaṃ piṇḍa-svedopanāhanam ।।

granthi-visarpa-śūle tu tailenoṣṇena secayet ।
daśa-mūla-vipakvena tad-van mūtrair jalena vā ।।

sukhoṣṇayā pradihyād vā piṣṭayā kṛṣṇagandhayā ।
naktamāla-tvacā śuṣka-mūlakaiḥ kalinātha-vā ।।

dantī citraka-mūla-tvak saudhārka-payasī guḍaḥ ।
bhallātakāsthi kāsīsaṃ lepo bhindyāc chilām api ।।

nuhy-arka-payasī guḍaḥ
bahir-mārgāśritaṃ granthiṃ kiṃ punaḥ kapha-saṃbhavam ।
dīrgha-kāla-sthitaṃ granthim ebhir bhindyāc ca bheṣajaiḥ ।।

mūlakānāṃ kulatthānāṃ yūṣaiḥ sa-kṣāra-dāḍimaiḥ ।
godhūmānnair yavānnair vā sa-sīdhu-madhu-śārkaraiḥ ।।

odhūmānnair yavānnaiś ca a-sīdhu-madhu-śarkaraiḥ
sa-kṣaudrair vāruṇī-maṇḍair mātuluṅga-rasānvitaiḥ ।
tri-phalāyāḥ prayogaiś ca pippalyāḥ kṣaudra-saṃyutaiḥ ।।

ippalī-kṣaudra-saṃyutaiḥ
devadāru-guḍūcyoś ca prayogair girijasya ca ।
musta-bhallāta-saktūnāṃ prayogair mākṣikasya ca ।।

dhūmair virekaiḥ śirasaḥ pūrvoktair gulma-bhedanaiḥ ।
taptāyo-hema-lavaṇa-pāṣāṇādi-prapīḍanaiḥ ।।

ābhiḥ kriyābhiḥ siddhābhir vividhābhir bale sthitaḥ ।
granthiḥ pāṣāṇa-kaṭhino yadi naivopaśāmyati ।।

athāsya dāhaḥ kṣāreṇa śarair hemnāpi vā hitaḥ ।
pākibhiḥ pācayitvā vā pāṭayitvā tam uddharet ।।

ākibhiḥ pācayitvā ca
mokṣayed bahu-śaś cāsya raktam utkleśam āgatam ।
punaś cāpahṛte rakte vāta-śleṣma-jid auṣadham ।।

praklinne dāha-pākābhyāṃ bāhyāntar vraṇa-vat kriyā ।
dārvī-viḍaṅga-kampillaiḥ siddhaṃ tailaṃ vraṇe hitam ।।

dūrvā-sva-rasa-siddhaṃ tu kapha-pittottare ghṛtam ।
ekataḥ sarva-karmāṇi rakta-mokṣaṇam ekataḥ ।।

visarpo na hy a-saṃsṛṣṭaḥ sa asra-pittena jāyate ।
raktam evāśrayaś cāsya bahu-śo asraṃ hared ataḥ ।।

na ghṛtaṃ bahu-doṣāya deyaṃ yan na virecanam ।
tena doṣo hy upastabdhas tvag-rakta-piśitaṃ pacet ।।

cikitsāsthāna
kuṣṭhinaṃ sneha-pānena pūrvaṃ sarvam upācaret ।
tatra vātottare tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā sādhitaṃ hitam ।।

daśa-mūlāmṛtairaṇḍa-śārṅgaṣṭā-meṣaśṛṅgibhiḥ ।
paṭola-nimba-kaṭukā-dārvī-pāṭhā-durālabhāḥ ।।

parpaṭaṃ trāyamāṇāṃ ca palāṃśaṃ pācayed apām ।
dvy-āḍhake aṣṭāṃśa-śeṣeṇa tena karṣonmitais tathā ।।

trāyantī-musta-bhūnimba-kaliṅga-kaṇa-candanaiḥ ।
sarpiṣo dvā-daśa-palaṃ pacet tat tiktakaṃ jayet ।।

pitta-kuṣṭha-parīsarpa-piṭikā-dāha-tṛḍ-bhramān ।
kaṇḍū-pāṇḍv-āmayān gaṇḍān duṣṭa-nāḍī-vraṇāpacīḥ ।।

visphoṭa-vidradhī-gulma-śophonmāda-madān api ।
hṛd-roga-timira-vyaṅga-grahaṇī-śvitra-kāmalāḥ ।।

bhagandaram apasmāram udaraṃ pradaraṃ garam ।
arśo-'sra-pittam anyāṃś ca su-kṛcchrān pitta-jān gadān ।।

sa-pracchadaḥ parpaṭakaḥ śamyākaḥ kaṭukā vacā ।
tri-phalā padmakaṃ pāṭhā rajanyau śārive kaṇe ।।

nimba-candana-yaṣṭy-āhva-viśālendrayavāmṛtāḥ ।
kirātatiktakaṃ sevyaṃ vṛṣo mūrvā śatāvarī ।।

paṭolātiviṣā-mustā-trāyantī-dhanvayāsakam ।
tair jale aṣṭa-guṇe sarpir dvi-guṇāmalakī-rase ।।

siddhaṃ tiktān mahā-tiktaṃ guṇair abhyadhikaṃ matam ।
kaphottare ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ nimba-saptāhva-citrakaiḥ ।।

kuṣṭhoṣaṇa-vacā-śāla-priyāla-caturaṅgulaiḥ ।
sarveṣu cāruṣkara-jaṃ taubaraṃ sārṣapaṃ pibet ।।

snehaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā kṛmijit-pathyā-bhallātakaiḥ śṛtam ।
āragvadhasya mūlena śata-kṛtvaḥ śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।।

-pathyā-bhallātaka-śṛtam apta-kṛtvaḥ śṛtaṃ ghṛtam
piban kuṣṭhaṃ jayaty āśu bhajan sa-khadiraṃ jalam ।
ebhir eva yathā-svaṃ ca snehair abhyañjanaṃ hitam ।।

ibet kuṣṭhaṃ jayaty āśu
snigdhasya śodhanaṃ yojyaṃ visarpe yad udāhṛtam ।
lalāṭa-hasta-pādeṣu sirāś cāsya vimokṣayet ।।

pracchānam alpake kuṣṭhe śṛṅgādyāś ca yathā-yatham ।
snehair āpyāyayec cainaṃ kuṣṭha-ghnair antarāntarā ।।

mukta-rakta-viriktasya rikta-koṣṭhasya kuṣṭhinaḥ ।
prabhañjanas tathā hy asya na syād deha-prabhañjanaḥ ।।

vāsāmṛtā-nimba-varā-paṭola-vyāghrī-karañjodaka-kalka-pakvam ।
sarpir visarpa-jvara-kāmalāsra-kuṣṭhāpahaṃ vajrakam āmananti ।।

tri-phalā-tri-kaṭu-dvi-kaṇṭakārī-kaṭukā-kumbha-nikumbha-rājavṛkṣaiḥ ।
sa-vacātiviṣāgnikaiḥ sa-pāṭhaiḥ picu-bhāgair nava-vajra-dugdha-muṣṭyā ।।

piṣṭaiḥ siddhaṃ sarpiṣaḥ prastham ebhiḥ krūre koṣṭhe snehanaṃ recanaṃ ca ।
kuṣṭha-śvitra-plīha-vardhmāśma-gulmān hanyāt kṛcchrāṃs tan mahā-vajrakākhyam ।। 

।।

danty-āḍhakam apāṃ droṇe paktvā tena ghṛtaṃ pacet ।
dhāmārgava-pale pītaṃ tad ūrdhvādho viśuddhi-kṛt ।।

āvartakī-tulāṃ droṇe paced aṣṭāṃśa-śeṣitam ।
tan-mūlais tatra niryūhe ghṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।।

pītvā tad eka-divasāntaritaṃ su-jīrṇe bhuñjīta kodravam a-saṃskṛta-kāñjikena ।
kuṣṭhaṃ kilāsam apacīṃ ca vijetum icchan icchan prajāṃ ca vipulāṃ grahaṇaṃ smṛtiṃ ca ।।

।।

huñjīta kodrava-su-saṃskṛta-kāñjikena
yater lelītaka-vasā kṣaudra-jātī-rasānvitā ।
kuṣṭha-ghnī sama-sarpir vā sa-gāyatry-asanodakā ।।

śālayo yava-godhūmāḥ koradūṣāḥ priyaṅgavaḥ ।
mudgā masūrās tubarī tikta-śākāni jāṅgalam ।।

varā-paṭola-khadira-nimbāruṣkara-yojitam ।
madyāny auṣadha-garbhāṇi mathitaṃ cendurāji-mat ।।

anna-pānaṃ hitaṃ kuṣṭhe na tv amla-lavaṇoṣaṇam ।
dadhi-dugdha-guḍānūpa-tila-māṣāṃs tyajet-tarām ।।

paṭola-mūla-tri-phalā-viśālāḥ pṛthak-tri-bhāgāpacita-tri-śāṇāḥ ।
syus trāyamāṇā kaṭu-rohiṇī ca bhāgārdhike nāgara-pāda-yukte ।।

etat palaṃ jarjaritaṃ vipakvaṃ jale pibed doṣa-viśodhanāya ।
jīrṇe rasair dhanva-mṛga-dvi-jānāṃ purāṇa-śāly-odanam ādadīta ।।

kuṣṭhaṃ kilāsaṃ grahaṇī-pradoṣam arśāṃsi kṛcchrāṇi halīmakaṃ ca ।
ṣaḍ-rātra-yogena nihanti caitad hṛd-vasti-śūlaṃ viṣama-jvaraṃ ca ।।

ṣaḍ-rātra-yogena nihanti caiṣa
viḍaṅga-sārāmalakābhayānāṃ pala-trayaṃ trīṇi palāni kumbhāt ।
guḍasya ca dvā-daśa māsam eṣa jitātmanāṃ hanty upayujymānaḥ ।।

kuṣṭha-śvitra-śvāsa-kāsodarārśo-meha-plīha-granthi-rug-jantu-gulmān ।
siddhaṃ yogaṃ prāha yakṣo mumukṣor bhikṣoḥ prāṇān māṇibhadraḥ kilemam ।।

bhūnimba-nimba-tri-phalā-padmakātiviṣā-kaṇāḥ ।
mūrvā-paṭolī-dvi-niśā-pāṭhā-tiktendravāruṇīḥ ।।

sa-kaliṅga-vacās tulyā dvi-guṇāś ca yathottaram ।
lihyād dantī-trivṛd-brāhmīs cūrṇitā madhu-sarpiṣā ।।

kuṣṭha-meha-prasuptīnāṃ paramaṃ syāt tad auṣadham ।
varā-viḍaṅga-kṛṣṇā vā lihyāt tailājya-mākṣikaiḥ ।।

uṣṭha-meha-prataptānāṃ
kākodumbarikā-vella-nimbābda-vyoṣa-kalka-vān ।
hanti vṛkṣaka-niryūhaḥ pānāt sarvāṃs tvag-āmayān ।।

ānāt sarva-tvag-āmayān
kuṭajāgni-nimba-nṛpataru-khadirāsana-saptaparṇa-niryūhe ।
siddhā madhu-ghṛta-yuktāḥ kuṣṭha-ghnīr bhakṣayed abhayāḥ ।।
dārvī-khadira-nimbānāṃ tvak-kvāthaḥ kuṣṭha-sūdanaḥ ।।
niśottamā-nimba-paṭola-mūla-tiktā-vacā-lohitayaṣṭikābhiḥ ।
kṛtaḥ kaṣāyaḥ kapha-pitta-kuṣṭhaṃ su-sevito dharma ivocchinatti ।।

ebhir eva ca śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ukhyaṃ bheṣajair jayati māruta-kuṣṭham ।
kalpayet khadira-nimba-guḍūcī-devadāru-rajanīḥ pṛthag evam ।।
pāṭhā-dārvī-vahni-ghuṇeṣṭā-kaṭukābhir ।।mūtraṃ yuktaṃ śakrayavaiś coṣṇa-jalaṃ vā ।।kuṣṭhī pītvā māsam a-ruk syād guda-kīlī ।।mehī śophī pāṇḍura-jīrṇī kṛmi-māṃś ca ।।lākṣā-dantī-madhurasa-varā-dvīpi-pāṭhā-viḍaṅga- ।।
ākṣā-dantī-madhurasa-varā-dvīpi-pāṭhā-viḍaṅgaṃ -pratyakpuṣpī-tri-kaṭu-rajanī-saptaparṇāṭarūṣam ।।

ratyakpuṣpī-tri-kaṭu-rajanī-saptaparṇāṭarūṣam raktā nimbaṃ surataru kṛtaṃ pañca-mūlyau ca cūrṇaṃ ।।
pītvā māsaṃ jayati hita-bhug gavya-mūtreṇa kuṣṭham ।।
niśā-kaṇā-nāgara-vella-taubaraṃ sa-vahni-tāpyaṃ krama-śo vivardhitam ।
gavāmbu-pītaṃ vaṭakī-kṛtaṃ tathā nihanti kuṣṭhāni sa-dāruṇāny api ।।

tri-kaṭūttamā-tilāruṣkarājya-mākṣika-sitopalā-vihitā ।
guṭikā rasāyanaṃ kuṣṭha-jic ca vṛṣyā ca sapta-samā ।।

uṭikā rasāyanaṃ syāt c ṃṭha-hṛc ca vṛṣyā ca sapta-samā 
uṣṭha-jic ca vṛṣyā ca sapta-samā
candraśakalāgni-rajanī-viḍaṅga-tubarāsthy-aruṣkara-tri-phalābhiḥ ।
vaṭakā guḍāṃśa-kḷptāḥ samasta-kuṣṭhāni nāśayanty abhyastāḥ ।।

viḍaṅga-bhallātaka-vākucīnāṃ sa-dvīpi-vārāhi-harītakīnām ।
sa-lāṅgalī-kṛṣṇa-tilopakulyā guḍena piṇḍī vinihanti kuṣṭham ।।

śaśāṅkalekhā sa-viḍaṅga-sārā sa-pippalīkā sa-hutāśa-mūlā ।
sāyo-malā sāmalakā sa-tailā kuṣṭhāni kṛcchrāṇi nihanti līḍhā ।।

śaśāṅkalekhā sa-viḍaṅga-mūlā
pathyā-tila-guḍaiḥ piṇḍī kuṣṭhaṃ sāruṣkarair jayet ।
guḍāruṣkara-jantughna-somarājī-kṛtātha-vā ।।

viḍaṅgādri-jatu-kṣaudra-sarpiṣ-mat khādiraṃ rajaḥ ।
kiṭibha-śvitra-dadrū-ghnaṃ khāden mita-hitāśanaḥ ।।

sitā-taila-kṛmighnāni dhātry-ayo-mala-pippalīḥ ।
lihānaḥ sarva-kuṣṭhāni jayaty ati-gurūṇy api ।।

mustaṃ vyoṣaṃ tri-phalā mañjiṣṭhā dāru pañca-mūle dve ।
saptacchada-nimba-tvak sa-viśālā citrako mūrvā ।।

cūrṇaṃ tarpaṇa-bhāgair navabhiḥ saṃyojitaṃ sa-madhv-aṃśam ।
nityaṃ kuṣṭha-nibarhaṇam etat prāyogikaṃ khādan ।।

śvayathuṃ sa-pāṇḍu-rogaṃ śvitraṃ grahaṇī-pradoṣam arśāṃsi ।
vardhma-bhagandara-piṭikā-kaṇḍū-koṭhāpacīr hanti ।।

rasāyana-prayogeṇa tubarāsthīni śīlayet ।
bhallātakaṃ vākucikāṃ vahni-mūlaṃ śilāhvayam ।।

iti doṣe vijite antas-tvak-sthe śamanaṃ bahiḥ pralepādi hitam ।
tīkṣṇālepotkliṣṭaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hi vivṛddhim eti maline dehe ।।

sthira-kaṭhina-maṇḍalānāṃ kuṣṭhānāṃ poṭalair hitaḥ svedaḥ ।
svinnotsannaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śastrair likhitaṃ pralepanair limpet ।।

yeṣu na śastraṃ kramate sparśendriya-nāśaneṣu kuṣṭheṣu ।
teṣu nipātyaḥ kṣāro raktaṃ doṣaṃ ca visrāvya ।।

lepo ati-kaṭhina-paruṣe supte kuṣṭhe sthire purāṇe ca ।
pītā-gadasya kāryo viṣaiḥ sa-mantro a-gadaiś cānu ।।

iṣaiḥ sa-mantrā-gadaiś cānu
stabdhāni supta-suptāny a-svedana-kaṇḍulāni kuṣṭhāni ।
ghṛṣṭāni śuṣka-go-maya-phenaka-śastraiḥ pradehyāni ।।

mustā tri-phalā madanaṃ karañja āragvadhaḥ kaliṅga-yavāḥ ।
saptāhva-kuṣṭha-phalinī-dārvyaḥ siddhārthakaṃ snānam ।।

eṣa kaṣāyo vamanaṃ virecanaṃ varṇakas tathodgharṣaḥ ।
tvag-doṣa-kuṣṭha-śopha-prabādhanaḥ pāṇḍu-roga-ghnaḥ ।।

karavīra-nimba-kuṭajāc chamyākāc citrakāc ca mūlānām ।
mūtre darvī-lepī kvātho lepena kuṣṭha-ghnaḥ ।।

śveta-karavīra-mūlaṃ kuṭaja-karañjāt phalaṃ tvaco dārvyāḥ ।
sumanaḥ-pravāla-yukto lepaḥ kuṣṭhāpahaḥ siddhaḥ ।।

śairīṣī tvak puṣpaṃ kārpāsyā rājavṛkṣa-pattrāṇi ।
piṣṭā ca kākamācī catur-vidhaḥ kuṣṭha-hā lepaḥ ।।

vyoṣa-sarṣapa-niśā-gṛha-dhūmair yāva-śūka-paṭu-citraka-kuṣṭhaiḥ ।
kola-mātra-guṭikārdha-viṣāṃśā śvitra-kuṣṭha-haraṇo vara-lepaḥ ।।

nimbaṃ haridre surasaṃ paṭolaṃ kuṣṭhāśvagandhe suradāru śigruḥ ।
sa-sarṣapaṃ tumburu-dhānya-vanyaṃ caṇḍā ca cūrṇāni samāni kuryāt ।।

tais takra-piṣṭaiḥ prathamaṃ śarīraṃ tailāktam udvartayituṃ yateta ।
tathāsya kaṇḍūḥ piṭikāḥ sa-koṭhāḥ kuṣṭhāni śophāś ca śamaṃ vrajanti ।।

enāsya kaṇḍūḥ piṭikāḥ sa-koṭhāḥ
mustāmṛtāsaṅga-kaṭaṅkaṭerī-kāsīsa-kampillaka-kuṣṭha-lodhrāḥ ।
gandhopalaḥ sarja-raso viḍaṅgaṃ manaḥśilāle karavīraka-tvak ।।

tailākta-gātrasya kṛtāni cūrṇāny etāni dadyād avacūrṇanārtham ।
dadrūḥ sa-kaṇḍūḥ kiṭibhāni pāmā vicarcikā ceti tathā na santi ।।

snug-gaṇḍe sarṣapāt kalkaḥ kukūlānala-pācitaḥ ।
lepād vicarcikāṃ hanti rāga-vega iva trapām ।।

manaḥśilāle maricāni tailam ārkaṃ payaḥ kuṣṭha-haraḥ pradehaḥ ।
tathā karañja-prapunāṭa-bījaṃ kuṣṭhānvitaṃ go-salilena piṣṭam ।।

guggulu-marica-viḍaṅgaiḥ sarṣapa-kāsīsa-sarja-rasa-mustaiḥ ।
śrīveṣṭa-kālagandhair manaḥśilā-kuṣṭha-kampillaiḥ ।।

ubhaya-haridrā-sahitaiś cākrika-tailena miśritair ebhiḥ ।
dina-kara-karābhitaptaiḥ kuṣṭhaṃ ghṛṣṭaṃ ca naṣṭaṃ ca ।।

maricaṃ tamāla-pattraṃ kuṣṭhaṃ sa-manaḥśilaṃ sa-kāsīsam ।
tailena yuktam uṣitaṃ saptāhaṃ bhājane tāmre ।।

tenāliptaṃ sidhmaṃ saptāhād gharma-sevino apaiti ।
māsān navaṃ kilāsaṃ snānena vinā viśuddhasya ।।

mayūraka-kṣāra-jale sapta-kṛtvaḥ parisrute ।
siddhaṃ jyotiṣmatī-tailam abhyaṅgāt sidhma-nāśanam ।।

vāyasajaṅghā-mūlaṃ vamanī-pattrāṇi mūlakād bījam ।
takreṇa bhauma-vāre lepaḥ sidhmāpahaḥ siddhaḥ ।।

jīvantī mañjiṣṭhā dārvī kampillakaṃ payas tuttham ।
eṣa ghṛta-taila-pākaḥ siddhaḥ siddhe ca sarja-rasaḥ ।।

deyaḥ sa-madhūcchiṣṭo vipādikā tena naśyati hy aktā ।
carmaika-kuṣṭha-kiṭibhaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śāmyaty alasakaṃ ca ।।

mūlaṃ saptāhvāt tvak śirīṣāśvamārād arkān mālatyāś citrakāsphota-nimbāt ।
bījaṃ kārañjaṃ sārṣapaṃ prāpunāṭam śreṣṭhā jantughnaṃ try-ūṣaṇaṃ dve haridre ।।

tailaṃ tailaṃ sādhitaṃ taiḥ sa-mūtrais tvag-doṣāṇāṃ duṣṭa-nāḍī-vraṇānām ।
abhyaṅgena śleṣma-vātodbhavānāṃ nāśāyālaṃ vajrakaṃ vajra-tulyam ।।
eraṇḍa-tārkṣya-ghana-nīpa-kadamba-bhārgī- ।।-kampilla-vella-phalinī-suravāruṇībhiḥ ।।nirguṇḍy-aruṣkara-surāhva-suvarṇadugdhā- ।।-śrīveṣṭa-guggulu-śilā-paṭu-tāla-viśvaiḥ ।।
tulya-snug-arka-dugdhaṃ siddhaṃ tailaṃ smṛtaṃ mahā-vajram ।
atiśayita-vajraka-guṇaṃ śvitrārśo-granthi-mālā-ghnam ।।

kuṣṭhāśvamāra-bhṛṅgārka-mūtra-snuk-kṣīra-saindhavaiḥ ।
tailaṃ siddhaṃ viṣāpaham abhyaṅgāt kuṣṭha-jit param ।।

siddhaṃ sikthaka-sindūra-pura-tutthaka-tārkṣya-jaiḥ ।
kacchūṃ vicarcikāṃ cāśu kaṭu-tailaṃ nibarhati ।।

-pura-tutthaka-tārkṣyakaiḥ āmāṃ vicarcikāṃ cāśu 
kaṭu-tailaṃ niyacchati
lākṣā vyoṣaṃ prāpunāṭaṃ ca bījaṃ sa-śrīveṣṭaṃ kuṣṭha-siddhārthakāś ca ।
takronmiśraḥ syād dharidrā ca lepo dadrūṣūkto mūlakotthaṃ ca bījam ।।

citraka-śobhāñjanakau guḍūcy-apāmārga-devadārūṇi ।
khadiro dhavaś ca lepaḥ śyāmā dantī dravantī ca ।।

lākṣā-rasāñjanailāḥ punarnavā ceti kuṣṭhināṃ lepāḥ ।
dadhi-maṇḍa-yutāḥ pādaiḥ ṣaṭ proktā māruta-kapha-ghnāḥ ।।

jala-vāpya-loha-kesara-pattra-plava-candana-mṛṇālāni ।
bhāgottarāṇi siddhaṃ pralepanaṃ pitta-kapha-kuṣṭhe ।।

tikta-ghṛtair dhauta-ghṛtair abhyaṅgo dahyamāna-kuṣṭheṣu ।
tailaiś candana-madhuka-prapauṇḍarīkotpala-yutaiś ca ।।

klede prapatati cāṅge dāhe visphoṭake ca carma-dale ।
śītāḥ pradeha-sekā vyadhana-virekau ghṛtaṃ tiktam ।।

khadira-vṛṣa-nimba-kuṭajāḥ śreṣṭhā-kṛmijit-paṭola-madhuparṇyaḥ ।
antar bahiḥ prayuktāḥ kṛmi-kuṣṭha-nudaḥ sa-go-mutrāḥ ।।

pralepodvartana-snāna-pāna-bhojana-karmaṇi ।
śīlitaṃ khādiraṃ vāri sarva-tvag-doṣa-nāśanam ।।

vātottareṣu sarpir vamanaṃ śleṣmottareṣu kuṣṭheṣu ।
pittottareṣu mokṣo raktasya virecanaṃ cāgre ।।

aktasya virecanaṃ cāgryam
ye lepāḥ kuṣṭhānāṃ yujyante nirhṛtāsra-doṣāṇām ।
saṃśodhitāśayānāṃ sadyaḥ siddhir bhavati teṣām ।।

doṣe hṛte apanīte rakte bāhyāntare kṛte śamane ।
snehe ca kāla-yukte na kuṣṭham ativartate sādhyam ।।

bahu-doṣaḥ saṃśodhyaḥ kuṣṭhī bahu-śo anurakṣatā prāṇān ।
doṣe hy ati-mātra-hṛte vāyur hanyād a-balam āśu ।।

pakṣāt pakṣāc chardanāny abhyupeyān māsān māsāc chodhanāny apy adhas-tāt ।
śuddhir mūrdhni syāt tri-rātrāt tri-rātrāt ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe māsy asṛṅ-mokṣaṇaṃ ca ।।

ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe māsy asṛṅ-mokṣaṇāni yo dur-vānto dur-virikto atha-vā syāt ।।
kuṣṭhī doṣair uddhatair vyāpyate asau ।।niḥ-saṃdehaṃ yāty a-sādhya-tvam evaṃ ।।tasmāt kṛtsnān nirhared asya doṣān ।।vrata-dama-yama-sevā-tyāga-śīlābhiyogo ।।dvi-ja-sura-guru-pūjā sarva-sat-tveṣu maitrī ।।śiva-śiva-suta-tārā-bhās-karārādhanāni ।।
ina-jina-suta-tārā-bhās-karārādhanāni prakaṭita-mala-pāpaṃ kuṣṭham unmūlayanti ।।

cikitsāsthāna
kuṣṭhād api bībhatsaṃ yac chīghra-taraṃ ca yāty a-sādhya-tvam ।
śvitram atas tac-chāntyai yateta dīpte yathā bhavane ।।

saṃśodhanaṃ viśeṣāt prayojayet pūrvam eva dehasya ।
śvitre sraṃsanam agryaṃ malayū-rasa iṣyate sa-guḍaḥ ।।

taṃ pītvābhyakta-tanur yathā-balaṃ sūrya-pāda-saṃtāpam ।
seveta virikta-tanur try-ahaṃ pipāsuḥ pibet peyām ।।

śvitre aṅge ye sphoṭā jāyante kaṇṭakena tān bhindyāt ।
sphoṭeṣu niḥsruteṣu prātaḥ prātaḥ pibet tri-dinam ।।

rātaḥ prātaḥ pibet pakṣam
malayūm asanaṃ priyaṅguṃ śatapuṣpāṃ cāmbhasā samutkvāthya ।
pālāśaṃ vā kṣāraṃ yathā-balaṃ phāṇitopetam ।।

phalgv-akṣa-vṛkṣa-valkala-niryūheṇendurājikā-kalkam ।
pītvoṣṇa-sthitasya jāte sphoṭe takreṇa bhojanaṃ nir-lavaṇam ।।

gavyaṃ mūtraṃ citraka-vyoṣa-yuktaṃ sarpiḥ-kumbhe sthāpitaṃ kṣaudra-miśram ।
pakṣād ūrdhvaṃ śvitriṇā peyam etat kāryaṃ cāsmai kuṣṭha-diṣṭaṃ vidhānam ।।

akṣād ūrdhvaṃ śvitribhiḥ peyam etat
mārkavam atha-vā svāded bhṛṣṭaṃ tailena loha-pātra-stham ।
bījaka-śṛtaṃ ca dugdhaṃ tad anu pibec chvitra-nāśāya ।।

pūtīkārka-vyādhighāta-snuhīnāṃ mūtre piṣṭāḥ pallavā jāti-jāś ca ।
ghnanty ālepāc chvitra-dur-nāma-dadrū-pāmā-koṭhān duṣṭa-nāḍī-vraṇāṃś ca ।।

dvaipaṃ dagdhaṃ carma mātaṅga-jaṃ vā śvitre lepas taila-yukto variṣṭhaḥ ।
pūtiḥ kīṭo rājavṛkṣodbhavena kṣāreṇāktaḥ śvitram eko api hanti ।।

ṣāreṇāktaḥ śvitram eko nihanti
rātrau go-mūtre vāsitān jarjarāṅgān ahni cchāyāyāṃ śoṣayet sphoṭa-hetūn ।
evaṃ vārāṃs trīṃs tais tataḥ ślakṣṇa-piṣṭaiḥ snuhyāḥ kṣīreṇa śvitra-nāśāya lepaḥ ।। 

।।

akṣa-taila-drutā lepaḥ kṛṣṇa-sarpodbhavā maṣī ।
śikhi-pittaṃ tathā dagdhaṃ hrīveraṃ vā tad-āplutam ।।

kṣa-taila-kṛto lepaḥ kṣa-taila-druto lepaḥ
kuḍavo avalguja-bījād dharitāla-catur-bhāga-saṃmiśraḥ ।
mūtreṇa gavāṃ piṣṭaḥ sa-varṇa-karaṇaṃ paraṃ śvitre ।।

kṣāre su-dagdhe gaja-liṇḍa-je ca gajasya mūtreṇa parisrute ca ।
droṇa-pramāṇe daśa-bhāga-yuktaṃ dattvā paced bījam avalgujānām ।।

ṣāre su-dagdhe gaja-liṇḍa-je vā ajasya mūtre ca parisrute ca
śvitraṃ jayec cikkaṇa-tāṃ gatena tena pralimpan bahu-śaḥ praghṛṣṭaṃ ।
kuṣṭhaṃ maṣaṃ vā tila-kālakaṃ vā yad vā vraṇe syād adhi-māṃsa-jātam ।।

bhallātakaṃ dvīpi-sudhārka-mūlaṃ guñjā-phalaṃ try-ūṣaṇa-śaṅkha-cūrṇam ।
tutthaṃ sa-kuṣṭhaṃ lavaṇāni pañca kṣāra-dvayaṃ lāṅgalikāṃ ca paktvā ।।

hallātaka-dvīpi-sudhārka-mūla- 
-guñjā-phala-try-ūṣaṇa-śaṅkha-cūrṇam
snug-arka-dugdhe ghanam āyasa-sthaṃ śalākayā tad vidadhīta lepam ।
kuṣṭhe kilāse tila-kālakeṣu maṣeṣu dur-nāmasu carma-kīle ।।

śuddhyā śoṇita-mokṣair virūkṣaṇair bhakṣaṇaiś ca saktūnām ।
śvitraṃ kasya-cid eva praśāmyati kṣīṇa-pāpasya ।।

snigdha-svinne guḍa-kṣīra-matsyādyaiḥ kṛmiṇodare ।
utkleśita-kṛmi-kaphe śarvarīṃ tāṃ sukhoṣite ।।

surasādi-gaṇaṃ mūtre kvāthayitvārdha-vāriṇi ।
taṃ kaṣāyaṃ kaṇā-gāla-kṛmijit-kalka-yojitam ।।

sa-taila-svarjikā-kṣāraṃ yuñjyād vastiṃ tato ahani ।
tasminn eva nirūḍhaṃ taṃ pāyayeta virecanam ।।

trivṛt-kalkaṃ phala-kaṇā-kaṣāyāloḍitaṃ tataḥ ।
ūrdhvādhaḥ-śodhite kuryāt pañca-kola-yutaṃ kramam ।।

kaṭu-tikta-kaṣāyāṇāṃ kaṣāyaiḥ pariṣecanam ।
kāle viḍaṅga-tailena tatas tam anuvāsayet ।।

aṣāyaiḥ pariṣecayet
śiro-roga-niṣedhoktam ācaren mūrdha-geṣv anu ।
udrikta-tikta-kaṭukam alpa-snehaṃ ca bhojanam ।।

lpa-snehaṃ ca bhojayet
viḍaṅga-kṛṣṇā-marica-pippalī-mūla-śigrubhiḥ ।
pibet sa-svarjikā-kṣārair yavāgūṃ takra-sādhitām ।।

iḍaṅga-kṛṣṇā-madhuka- ibet sa-svarjikā-kṣārāṃ
rasaṃ śirīṣa-kiṇihī-pāribhadraka-kembukāt ।
palāśa-bīja-pattūra-pūtikād vā pṛthak pibet ।।

sa-kṣaudraṃ surasādīn vā lihyāt kṣaudra-yutān pṛthak ।
śata-kṛtvo aśva-viṭ-cūrṇaṃ viḍaṅga-kvātha-bhāvitam ।।

kṛmi-mān madhunā lihyād bhāvitaṃ vā varā-rasaiḥ ।
śiro-gateṣu kṛmiṣu cūrṇaṃ pradhamanaṃ ca tat ।।

ākhukarṇī-kisalayaiḥ su-piṣṭaiḥ piṣṭa-miśritaiḥ ।
paktvā pūpalikāṃ khāded dhānyāmlaṃ ca pibed anu ।।

ākhuparṇī-kisalayaiḥ
sa-pañca-kola-lavaṇam a-sāndraṃ takram eva vā ।
nīpa-mārkava-nirguṇḍī-pallaveṣv apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।।

imbāpāmārga-nirguṇḍī-
viḍaṅga-cūrṇa-miśrair vā piṣṭair bhakṣyān prakalpayet ।
viḍaṅga-taṇḍulair yuktam ardhāṃśair ātape sthitam ।।

rdhāṃśair ātapa-sthitam
dinam āruṣkaraṃ tailaṃ pāne vastau ca yojayet ।
surāhva-sarala-snehaṃ pṛthag evaṃ ca kalpayet ।।

purīṣa-jeṣu su-tarāṃ dadyād vasti-virecane ।
śiro-virekaṃ vamanaṃ śamanaṃ kapha-janmasu ।।

rakta-jānāṃ pratīkāraṃ kuryāt kuṣṭha-cikitsitāt ।
indra-lupta-vidhiś cātra vidheyo roma-bhojiṣu ।।

kṣīrāṇi māṃsāni ghṛtaṃ guḍaṃ ca dadhīni śākāni ca parṇa-vanti ।
samāsato amlān madhurān rasāṃś ca kṛmīñ jihāsuḥ parivarjayeta ।।

cikitsāsthāna
kevalaṃ nir-upastambham ādau snehair upācaret ।
vāyuṃ sarpir-vasā-majja-taila-pānair naraṃ tataḥ ।।

sneha-klāntaṃ samāśvāsya payobhiḥ snehayet punaḥ ।
yūṣair grāmyaudakānūpa-rasair vā sneha-saṃyutaiḥ ।।

pāyasaiḥ kṛśaraiḥ sāmla-lavaṇaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ ।
nāvanais tarpaṇaiś cānnaiḥ su-snigdhaiḥ svedayet tataḥ ।।

sv-abhyaktaṃ sneha-saṃyuktaiḥ śaṅkarādyaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
snehāktaṃ svinnam aṅgaṃ tu vakraṃ stabdhaṃ sa-vedanam ।।

nehākta-svinnam aṅgaṃ tu
yatheṣṭam ānāmayituṃ sukham eva hi śakyate ।
śuṣkāṇy api hi kāṣṭhāni sneha-svedopapādanaiḥ ।।

neha-svedopanāhanaiḥ
śakyaṃ karmaṇya-tāṃ netuṃ kim u gātrāṇi jīvatām ।
harṣa-toda-rug-āyāma-śopha-stambha-grahādayaḥ ।।

svinnasyāśu praśāmyanti mārdavaṃ copajāyate ।
snehaś ca dhātūn saṃśuṣkān puṣṇāty āśūpayojitaḥ ।।

uṣṇāty āśu prayojitaḥ
balam agni-balaṃ puṣṭiṃ prāṇāṃś cāsyābhivardhayet ।
a-sakṛt taṃ punaḥ snehaiḥ svedaiś ca pratipādayet ।।

rāṇaṃ cāsyābhivardhayet
tathā sneha-mṛdau koṣṭhe na tiṣṭhanty anilāmayāḥ ।
yady etena sa-doṣa-tvāt karmaṇā na praśāmyati ।।

mṛdubhiḥ sneha-saṃyuktair bheṣajais taṃ viśodhayet ।
ghṛtaṃ tilvaka-siddhaṃ vā sātalā-siddham eva vā ।।

payasairaṇḍa-tailaṃ vā pibed doṣa-haraṃ śivam ।
snigdhāmla-lavaṇoṣṇādyair āhārair hi malaś citaḥ ।।

sroto baddhvānilaṃ rundhyāt tasmāt tam anulomayet ।
dur-balo yo a-virecyaḥ syāt taṃ nirūhair upācaret ।।

roto ruddhvānilaṃ rundhyāt
dīpanaiḥ pācanīyair vā bhojyair vā tad-yutair naram ।
saṃśuddhasyotthite cāgnau sneha-svedau punar hitau ।।

āmāśaya-gate vāyau vamita-pratibhojite ।
sukhāmbunā ṣaḍ-dharaṇaṃ vacādiṃ vā prayojayet ।।

ukhāmbunā ṣaṭ-caraṇaṃ
saṃdhukṣite agnau parato vidhiḥ kevala-vātikaḥ ।
matsyān nābhi-pradeśa-sthe siddhān bilva-śalāṭubhiḥ ।।

vasti-karma tv adho nābheḥ śasyate cāvapīḍakaḥ ।
koṣṭha-ge kṣāra-cūrṇādyā hitāḥ pācana-dīpanāḥ ।।

hṛt-sthe payaḥ sthirā-siddhaṃ śiro-vastiḥ śiro-gate ।
snaihikaṃ nāvanaṃ dhūmaḥ śrotrādīnāṃ ca tarpaṇam ।।

svedābhyaṅga-nivātāni hṛdyaṃ cānnaṃ tvag-āśrite ।
śītāḥ pradehā rakta-sthe vireko rakta-mokṣaṇam ।।

vedābhyaṅgāni śastāni
vireko māṃsa-medaḥ-sthe nirūhaḥ śamanāni ca ।
bāhyābhyantarataḥ snehair asthi-majja-gataṃ jayet ।।

praharṣo annaṃ ca śukra-sthe bala-śukra-karaṃ hitam ।
vibaddha-mārgaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu śukraṃ dadyād virecanam ।।

alyaṃ śukra-karaṃ hitam
viriktaṃ pratibhuktaṃ ca pūrvoktāṃ kārayet kriyām ।
garbhe śuṣke tu vātena bālānāṃ ca viśuṣyatām ।।

irikta-pratibhuktasya
sitā-kāśmarya-madhukaiḥ siddham utthāpane payaḥ ।
snāva-saṃdhi-sirā-prāpte sneha-dāhopanāhanam ।।

tailaṃ saṃkucite abhyaṅgo māṣa-saindhava-sādhitam ।
āgāra-dhūma-lavaṇa-tailair lepaḥ srute asṛji ।।

supte aṅge veṣṭa-yukte tu kartavyam upanāhanam ।
athāpatānakenārtam a-srastākṣam a-vepanam ।।

a-stabdha-meḍhram a-svedaṃ bahir-āyāma-varjitam ।
a-khaṭvāghātinaṃ cainaṃ tvaritaṃ samupācaret ।।

tatra prāg eva su-snigdha-svinnāṅge tīkṣṇa-nāvanam ।
sroto-viśuddhaye yuñjyād accha-pānaṃ tato ghṛtam ।।

vidāry-ādi-gaṇa-kvātha-dadhi-kṣīra-rasaiḥ śṛtam ।
nāti-mātraṃ tathā vāyur vyāpnoti sahasaiva vā ।।

kulattha-yava-kolāni bhadradārv-ādikaṃ gaṇam ।
niḥkvāthyānūpa-māṃsaṃ ca tenāmlaiḥ payasāpi ca ।।
