svādu-skandha-pratīvāpaṃ mahā-snehaṃ vipācayet ।
sekābhyaṅgāvagāhānna-pāna-nasyānuvāsanaiḥ ।।

sa hanti vātaṃ te te ca sneha-svedāḥ su-yojitāḥ ।
vegāntareṣu mūrdhānam a-sakṛc cāsya recayet ।।

avapīḍaiḥ pradhamanais tīkṣṇaiḥ śleṣma-nibarhaṇaiḥ ।
śvasanāsu vimuktāsu tathā saṃjñāṃ sa vindati ।।
sauvarcalābhayā-vyoṣa-siddhaṃ sarpiś cale adhike ।।
palāṣṭakaṃ tilvakato varāyāḥ prasthaṃ palāṃśaṃ guru-pañca-mūlam ।
sairaṇḍa-siṃhī-trivṛtaṃ ghaṭe apāṃ paktvā pacet pāda-śṛtena tena ।।

dadhnaḥ pātre yāva-śūkāt tri-bilvaiḥ sarpiḥ-prasthaṃ hanti tat sevyamānam ।
duṣṭān vātān eka-sarvāṅga-saṃsthān yoni-vyāpad-gulma-vardhmodaraṃ ca ।।

adhnaḥ pātre yāva-śūka-tri-bilvaiḥ vidhis tilvaka-vaj jñeyo ramyakāśokayor api ।।

śamyākāśokayor api
cikitsitam idaṃ kuryāc chuddha-vātāpatānake ।
saṃsṛṣṭa-doṣe saṃsṛṣṭaṃ cūrṇayitvā kaphānvite ।।

tumburūṇy abhayā hiṅgu pauṣkaraṃ lavaṇa-trayam ।
yava-kvāthāmbunā peyaṃ hṛt-pārśvārty-apatantrake ।।

hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ śuṇṭhī dāḍimaṃ sāmla-vetasam ।
pibed vā śleṣma-pavana-hṛd-rogoktaṃ ca śasyate ।।

āyāmayor ardita-vad bāhyābhyantarayoḥ kriyā ।
taila-droṇyāṃ ca śayanam āntaro atra su-dus-taraḥ ।।

vi-varṇa-danta-vadanaḥ srastāṅgo naṣṭa-cetanaḥ ।
prasvidyaṃś ca dhanuḥ-ṣkambhī daśa-rātraṃ na jīvati ।।

rasvidyaṃś ca dhanuḥ-stambhī
vegeṣv ato anya-thā jīven mandeṣu vinato jaḍaḥ ।
khañjaḥ kuṇiḥ pakṣa-hataḥ paṅgulo vikalo atha-vā ।।

aṅgulo vikalo api vā
hanu-sraṃse hanū snigdha-svinnau sva-sthānam ānayet ।
unnāmayec ca kuśalaś cibukaṃ vivṛtte mukhe ।।

nāmayet saṃvṛte śeṣam ekāyāma-vad ācaret ।
jihvā-stambhe yathāvasthaṃ kāryaṃ vāta-cikitsitam ।।

vāg-grahe koṣṇa-toyena vetasāmlaṃ piben naraḥ ।
mātuluṅga-rasaṃ tad-vad dhiṅgu-sauvarcalānvitam ।।

ardite nāvanaṃ mūrdhni tailaṃ śrotrākṣi-tarpaṇam ।
sa-śophe vamanaṃ dāha-rāga-yukte sirā-vyadhaḥ ।।

nava-nītena saṃyuktāṃ khāden māṣeṇḍarīṃ naraḥ ।
dur-vāram arditaṃ hanti saptāhān nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

snehanaṃ sneha-saṃyuktaṃ pakṣāghāte virecanam ।
ava-bāhau hitaṃ nasyaṃ snehaś cottara-bhaktikaḥ ।।

māṣa-balā-śuka-śimbī-kaṭtṛṇa-rāsnāśvagandhorubūkāṇām ।
kvātho nasya-nipīto rāmaṭha-lavaṇānvitaḥ koṣṇaḥ ।।

apanayati pakṣa-vātaṃ manyā-stambhaṃ sa-karṇa-nāda-rujam ।
dur-jayam ardita-vātaṃ saptāhāj jayati cāvaśyam ।।

guḍamañjaryā khapuraṃ vṛṣabhī-mūlaṃ ca śiśira-jala-piṣṭam ।
nāvana-vidhau prayojitam ava-bāhuka-gala-rujārti-haram ।।

daśa-mūla-balā-māṣa-kvāthaṃ tailājya-miśritam ।
sāyaṃ bhuktvā piben nasyaṃ viśvācyām ava-bāhuke ।।

ūru-stambhe tu na sneho na ca saṃśodhanaṃ hitam ।
śleṣmāma-medo-bāhulyād yuktyā tat-kṣapaṇāny ataḥ ।।

ūru-stambhe na ca sneho
kuryād rūkṣopacāraś ca yava-śyāmāka-kodravāḥ ।
śākair a-lavaṇaiḥ śastāḥ kiñ-cit-tailair jalaiḥ śṛtaiḥ ।।

jāṅgalair a-ghṛtair māṃsair madhv-ambho-'riṣṭa-pāyinaḥ ।
vatsakādir haridrādir vacādir vā sa-saindhavaḥ ।।

āḍhya-vāte sukhāmbhobhiḥ peyaḥ ṣaḍ-dharaṇo atha-vā ।
lihyāt kṣaudreṇa vā śreṣṭhā-cavya-tiktā-kaṇā-ghanāt ।।

āma-vāte sukhāmbhobhiḥ eyaḥ ṣaṭ-caraṇo atha-vā 
-cavya-tiktā-kaṇā-ghanān
citrakendrayavāḥ pāṭhā kaṭukātiviṣā niśā ।
vāta-vyādhi-praśamano yogaḥ ṣaḍ-dharaṇāhvayaḥ ।।

kalkaṃ sa-madhu vā cavya-pathyāgni-suradāru-jam ।
mūtrair vā śīlayet pathyāṃ gugguluṃ girisaṃbhavam ।।

vyoṣāgni-musta-tri-phalā-viḍaṅgair gugguluṃ samam ।
khādan sarvāñ jayed vyādhīn medaḥ-śleṣmāma-vāta-jān ।।

śāmyaty evaṃ kaphākrāntaḥ sa-medaskaḥ prabhañjanaḥ ।
kṣāra-mūtrānvitān svedān sekān udvartanāni ca ।।

kuryād dihyāc ca mūtrāḍhyaiḥ karañja-phala-sarṣapaiḥ ।
mūlair vāpy arka-tarkārī-nimba-jaiḥ sa-surāhvayaiḥ ।।

sa-kṣaudra-sarṣapā-pakva-loṣṭa-valmīka-mṛttikaiḥ ।
kapha-kṣayārthaṃ vyāyāme sahye cainaṃ pravartayet ।।

sthalāny ullaṅghayen nārīḥ śaktitaḥ pariśīlayet ।
sthira-toyaṃ saraḥ kṣemaṃ prati-sroto nadīṃ taret ।।

śleṣma-medaḥ-kṣaye cātra snehādīn avacārayet ।
sthāna-dūṣyādi cālocya kāryā śeṣeṣv api kriyā ।।

thānaṃ dūṣyādi cālocya
bṛhan-nimba-taror mūlaṃ vāriṇā paripeṣitam ।
saṃpītaṃ nāśayet kṣipram a-sādhyām api gṛdhrasīm ।।

tūṇī-pratūṇyor lavanaṃ sa-ghṛtaṃ kṣāra-hiṅgu vā ।
raktāvasecanaṃ kuryād abhīkṣṇaṃ vāta-kaṇṭake ।।

pibed eraṇḍa-tailaṃ vā dahet sūcībhir eva vā ।
sājyaiḥ saktubhir abhyaktau na cā-kṣīra-samanvitaiḥ ।।
śālmalī-tvag-viliptau vā pādau saṃtāpam udgataḥ ।।
sahacaraṃ suradāru sa-nāgaraṃ kvathitam ambhasi taila-vimiśritam ।
pavana-pīḍita-deha-gatiḥ piban druta-vilambita-go bhavatīcchayā ।।

rāsnā-mahauṣadha-dvīpi-pippalī-śaṭhi-pauṣkaram ।
piṣṭvā vipācayet sarpir vāta-roga-haraṃ param ।।

nimbāmṛtā-vṛṣa-paṭola-nidigdhikānāṃ bhāgān pṛthak daśa palān vipaced ghaṭe apām ।
aṣṭāṃśa-śeṣita-rasena punaś ca tena prasthaṃ ghṛtasya vipacet picu-bhāga-kalkaiḥ ।।

imbāmṛtā-vṛṣa-paṭola-karañjakānāṃ
pāṭhā-viḍaṅga-suradāru-gajopakulyā-dvi-kṣāra-nāgara-niśā-miśi-cavya-kuṣṭhaiḥ ।
tejovatī-marica-vatsaka-dīpyakāgni-rohiṇy-aruṣkara-vacā-kaṇa-mūla-yuktaiḥ ।।

mañjiṣṭhayātiviṣayā viṣayā yavānyā saṃśuddha-guggulu-palair api pañca-saṃkhyaiḥ । tat sevitaṃ vidhamati prabalaṃ samīraṃ saṃdhy-asthi-majja-gatam apy atha kuṣṭham īdṛk ।।

at sevitaṃ pradhamati prabalaṃ samīraṃ
nāḍī-vraṇārbuda-bhagandara-gaṇḍa-mālā-jatrūrdhva-sarva-gada-gulma-gudottha-mehān ।
yakṣmā-ruci-śvasana-pīnasa-kāsa-śopha-hṛt-pāṇḍu-roga-mada-vidradhi-vāta-raktam ।। 

।।

-hṛt-pārśva-roga-mada-vidradhi-vāta-raktam
rāsnāṭarūṣa-suradārv-amṛtā-śatāvary-eraṇḍa-puṣkara-dhamāsaka-śuṇṭhi-pathyāḥ ।
nighnanti vāta-ja-rujaṃ khalu sa-śvadaṃṣṭrāḥ śaileya-śaṭhy-ativiṣāḥ kvathitāḥ prayuktā ।।

।।

balā-bilva-śṛte kṣīre ghṛta-maṇḍaṃ vipācayet ।
tasya śuktiḥ prakuñco vā nasyaṃ vāte śiro-gate ।।

tad-vat siddhā vasā nakra-matsya-kūrma-culūka-jā ।
viśeṣeṇa prayoktavyā kevale mātariśvani ।।

jīrṇaṃ piṇyākaṃ pañca-mūlaṃ pṛthak ca kvāthyaṃ kvāthābhyām ekatas tailam ābhyām ।
kṣīrād aṣṭāṃśaṃ pācayet tena pānād vātā naśyeyuḥ śleṣma-yuktā viśeṣāt ।।

prasāriṇī-tulā-kvāthe taila-prasthaṃ payaḥ-samam ।
dvi-medā-miśi-mañjiṣṭhā-kuṣṭha-rāsnā-ku-candanaiḥ ।।

jīvakarṣabha-kākolī-yugalāmaradārubhiḥ ।
kalkitair vipacet sarva-mārutāmaya-nāśanam ।।

sa-mūla-śākhasya sahācarasya tulāṃ sametāṃ daśa-mūlataś ca ।
palāni pañcāśad abhīrutaś ca pādāvaśeṣaṃ vipaced vahe apām ।।

tatra sevya-nakha-kuṣṭha-himailā-spṛk-priyaṅgu-nalikāmbu-śilā-jaiḥ ।
lohitā-nalada-loha-surāhvaiḥ kopanā-miśi-turuṣka-nataiś ca ।।

tulya-kṣīraṃ pālikais taila-pātraṃ siddhaṃ kṛcchrāñ chīlitaṃ hanti vātān ।
kampākṣepa-stambha-śoṣādi-yuktān gulmonmādau pīnasaṃ yoni-rogān ।।

ulyaṃ kṣīraṃ pālikais taila-pātraṃ
sahacara-tulāyās tu rase tailāḍhakaṃ pacet ।
mūla-kalkād daśa-palaṃ payo dattvā catur-guṇam ।।

atha-vā nata-ṣaḍgranthā-sthirā-kuṣṭha-surāhvayāt ।
sailā-nalada-śaileya-śatāhvā-rakta-candanāt ।।

-sthirā-kuṣṭha-surāhvayān -śatāhvā-rakta-candanān
siddhe asmiñ charkarā-cūrṇād aṣṭā-daśa-palaṃ kṣipet ।
bheḍasya saṃmataṃ tailaṃ tat kṛcchrān anilāmayān ।।

vāta-kuṇḍalikonmāda-gulma-vardhmādikāñ jayet ।
balā-śataṃ chinnaruhā-pādaṃ rāsnāṣṭa-bhāgikam ।।

jalāḍhaka-śate paktvā śata-bhāga-sthite rase ।
dadhi-mastv-ikṣu-niryāsa-śuktais tailāḍhakaṃ samaiḥ ।।

pacet sāja-payo-'rdhāṃśaṃ kalkair ebhiḥ palonmitaiḥ ।
śaṭhī-saraladārv-elā-mañjiṣṭhāguru-candanaiḥ ।।

padmakātibalā-mustā-śūrpaparṇī-hareṇubhiḥ ।
yaṣṭy-āhva-surasa-vyāghranakharṣabhaka-jīvakaiḥ ।।

palāśa-rasa-kastūrī-nalikā-jāti-kośakaiḥ ।
spṛkkā-kuṅkuma-śaileya-jātī-kaṭuphalāmbubhiḥ ।।

-jātikā-kaṭphalāmbubhiḥ
tvak-kunduruka-karpūra-turuṣka-śrīnivāsakaiḥ ।
lavaṅga-nakha-kaṅkola-kuṣṭha-māṃsī-priyaṅgubhiḥ ।।

sthauṇeya-tagara-dhyāma-vacā-madanaka-plavaiḥ ।
sa-nāgakesaraiḥ siddhe dadyāc cātrāvatārite ।।

-vacā-madana-pallavaiḥ
pattra-kalkaṃ tataḥ pūtaṃ vidhinā tat prayojitam ।
kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ jvaraṃ chardiṃ mūrchāṃ gulma-kṣata-kṣayān ।।

plīha-śoṣāv apasmāram a-lakṣmīṃ ca praṇāśayet ।
balā-tailam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vāta-vyādhi-vināśanam ।।

pāne nasye anvāsane abhyañjane ca snehāḥ kāle samyag ete prayuktāḥ ।
duṣṭān vātān āśu śāntiṃ nayeyur vandhyā nārīḥ putra-bhājaś ca kuryuḥ ।।

andhyā nārīḥ putra-bhājaḥ prakuryuḥ
sneha-svedair drutaḥ śleṣmā yadā pakvāśaye sthitaḥ ।
pittaṃ vā darśayed rūpaṃ vastibhis taṃ vinirjayet ।।

adā pakvāśayaṃ sthitaḥ

cikitsāsthāna
vāta-śoṇitino raktaṃ snigdhasya bahu-śo haret ।
alpālpaṃ pālayan vāyuṃ yathā-doṣaṃ yathā-balam ।।

rug-rāga-toda-dāheṣu jalaukobhir vinirharet ।
śṛṅga-tumbaiś cimicimā-kaṇḍū-rug-dūyanānvitam ।।

pracchānena sirābhir vā deśād deśāntaraṃ vrajat ।
aṅga-glānau tu na srāvyaṃ rūkṣe vātottare ca yat ।।

ṅga-mlānau tu na srāvyaṃ ūkṣaṃ vātottaraṃ ca yat
gambhīraṃ śvayathuṃ stambhaṃ kampaṃ snāyu-sirāmayān ।
glānim anyāṃś ca vātotthān kuryād vāyur asṛk-kṣayāt ।।

virecyaḥ snehayitvā tu sneha-yuktair virecanaiḥ ।
vātottare vāta-rakte purāṇaṃ pāyayed ghṛtam ।।

śrāvaṇī-kṣīra-kākolī-kṣīriṇī-jīvakaiḥ samaiḥ ।
siddhaṃ sarṣabhakaiḥ sarpiḥ sa-kṣīraṃ vāta-rakta-nut ।।

drākṣā-madhūka-vāribhyāṃ siddhaṃ vā sa-sitopalam ।
ghṛtaṃ pibet tathā kṣīraṃ guḍūcī-sva-rase śṛtam ।।

tailaṃ payaḥ śarkarāṃ ca pāyayed vā su-mūrchitam ।
balā-śatāvarī-rāsnā-daśa-mūlaiḥ sa-pīlubhiḥ ।।

śyāmairaṇḍa-sthirābhiś ca vātārti-ghnaṃ śṛtaṃ payaḥ ।
dhāroṣṇaṃ mūtra-yuktaṃ vā kṣīraṃ doṣānulomanam ।।

paitte paktvā varī-tiktā-paṭola-tri-phalāmṛtāḥ ।
pibed ghṛtaṃ vā kṣīraṃ vā svādu-tiktaka-sādhitam ।।

kṣīreṇairaṇḍa-tailaṃ ca prayogeṇa piben naraḥ ।
bahu-doṣo virekārthaṃ jīrṇe kṣīraudanāśanaḥ ।।

kaṣāyam abhayānāṃ vā pāyayed ghṛta-bharjitam ।
kṣīrānu-pānaṃ trivṛtā-cūrṇaṃ drākṣā-rasena vā ।।

nirhared vā malaṃ tasya sa-ghṛtaiḥ kṣīra-vastibhiḥ ।
na hi vasti-samaṃ kiñ-cid vāta-rakta-cikitsitam ।।

viśeṣāt pāyu-pārśvoru-parvāsthi-jaṭharārtiṣu ।
mustā-dhātrī-haridrāṇāṃ pibet kvāthaṃ kapholbaṇe ।।

usta-drākṣā-haridrāṇāṃ
sa-kṣaudraṃ tri-phalāyā vā guḍūcīṃ vā yathā tathā ।
yathārha-sneha-pītaṃ ca vāmitaṃ mṛdu rūkṣayet ।।

uḍūcīṃ vā yathā-balam uḍūcīṃ vā yathā-yatham
tri-phalā-vyoṣa-pattrailā-tvakkṣīrī-citrakaṃ vacām ।
viḍaṅgaṃ pippalī-mūlaṃ romaśāṃ vṛṣakaṃ tvacam ।।

omaśaṃ vṛṣakaṃ tvacam
ṛddhiṃ lāṅgalikīṃ cavyaṃ sama-bhāgāni peṣayet ।
kalye liptvāyasīṃ pātrīṃ madhyāhne bhakṣayed idam ।।

vātāsre sarva-doṣe api paraṃ śūlānvite hitam ।
kokilākṣaka-niryūhaḥ pītas tac chāka-bhojinā ।।

ītas tac chāka-bhakṣiṇā
kṛpābhyāsa iva krodhaṃ vāta-raktaṃ niyacchati ।
pañca-mūlasya dhātryā vā rasair lelītakīṃ vasām ।।

khuḍaṃ su-rūḍham apy aṅge brahma-cārī piban jayet ।
ity ābhyantaram uddiṣṭaṃ karma bāhyam ataḥ param ।।

tri-phalāṣṭa-palaṃ kvāthya pāda-śeṣaṃ jalāḍhake ।
ṣo-ḍaśaiva palāny atra prakṣipec chuddha-gugguloḥ ।।

tatas tasmin ghanī-bhūte kalkī-kṛtya dvi-kārṣikāḥ ।
pathyā-viḍaṅga-kaṭukā guḍūcī pala-saṃmitā ।।

karṣāṃśe trivṛtā dantī khāded iṣṭānu-pānataḥ ।
vividham api vāta-raktaṃ sruta-śuṣka-sphuṭitam api hanti ।।

vraṇa-kāsa-kuṣṭha-gulma-śvayathūdara-pāṇḍu-meham arśāṃsi ।
abhibhūya jarā-doṣaṃ karoti kaiśorakaṃ kāyam ।।

āranālāḍhake tailaṃ pāda-sarja-rasaṃ śṛtam ।
prabhūte khajitaṃ toye jvara-dāhārti-nut param ।।

sa-madhūcchiṣṭa-mañjiṣṭhaṃ sa-sarja-rasa-śārivam ।
piṇḍa-tailaṃ tad abhyaṅgād vāta-rakta-rujāpaham ।।

daśa-mūla-śṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ sadyaḥ śūla-nivāraṇam ।
pariṣeko anila-prāye tad-vat koṣṇena sarpiṣā ।।

snehair madhura-siddhair vā caturbhiḥ pariṣecayet ।
stambhākṣepaka-śūlārtaṃ koṣṇair dāhe tu śītalaiḥ ।।

tad-vad gavyāvika-cchāgaiḥ kṣīrais taila-vimiśritaiḥ ।
niḥkvāthair jīvanīyānāṃ pañca-mūlasya vā laghoḥ ।।

drākṣekṣu-rasa-madyāni dadhi-mastv-amla-kāñjikam ।
sekārthaṃ taṇḍula-kṣaudra-śarkarāmbhaś ca śasyate ।।

priyāḥ priyaṃ-vadāḥ nāryāś candanārdra-kara-stanāḥ ।
sparśa-śītāḥ sukha-sparśā ghnanti dāhaṃ rujaṃ klamam ।।

sa-rāge sa-ruje dāhe raktaṃ hṛtvā pralepayet ।
prapauṇḍarīka-mañjiṣṭhā-dārvī-madhuka-candanaiḥ ।।

sitopalairakā-saktu-masūrośīra-padmakaiḥ ।
lepo rug-dāha-vīsarpa-rāga-śopha-nibarhaṇaḥ ।।

a-sitopala-kāsekṣu- -masūrairaka-saktubhiḥ
vāta-ghnaiḥ sādhitaḥ snigdhaḥ kṛśaro mudga-pāyasaḥ ।
tila-sarṣapa-piṇḍaiś ca śūla-ghnam upanāhanam ।।

ila-sarṣapa-piṇḍaś ca
audaka-prasahānūpa-vesavārāḥ su-saṃskṛtāḥ ।
jīvanīyauṣadhaiḥ sneha-yuktāḥ syur upanāhane ।।

īvanīyauṣadha-sneha-
stambha-toda-rug-āyāma-śophāṅga-graha-nāśanāḥ ।
jīvanīyauṣadhaiḥ siddhā sa-payaskā vasāpi vā ।।

ghṛtaṃ sahacarān mūlaṃ jīvantī chāgalaṃ payaḥ ।
lepaḥ piṣṭās tilās tad-vad bhṛṣṭāḥ payasi nirvṛtāḥ ।।

kṣīra-piṣṭa-kṣumāṃ lepam eraṇḍasya phalāni vā ।
kuryāc chūla-nivṛtty-arthaṃ śatāhvāṃ vānile adhike ।।

ṣīra-piṣṭām umāṃ lepam
mūtra-kṣāra-surā-pakvaṃ ghṛtam abhyañjane hitam ।
siddhaṃ sa-madhu śuktaṃ vā sekābhyaṅge kaphottare ।।

usta-kṣāra-sitā-pakvaṃ ekābhyaṅgaḥ kaphottare
gṛha-dhūmo vacā kuṣṭhaṃ śatāhvā rajanī-dvayam ।
pralepaḥ śūla-nud vāta-rakte vāta-kaphottare ।।

madhu-śigror hitaṃ tad-vad bījaṃ dhānyāmla-saṃyutam ।
muhūrta-liptam amlaiś ca siñced vāta-kaphottare ।।

uttānaṃ lepanābhyaṅga-pariṣekāvagāhanaiḥ ।
virekāsthāpana-sneha-pānair gambhīram ācaret ।।

vāta-śleṣmottare koṣṇā lepādyās tatra śītalaiḥ ।
vidāha-śopha-ruk-kaṇḍū-vivṛddhiḥ stambhanād bhavet ।।

pitta-raktottare vāta-rakte lepādayo himāḥ ।
uṣṇaiḥ ploṣoṣa-rug-rāga-svedāvadaraṇodbhavaḥ ।।

madhuyaṣṭyāḥ pala-śataṃ kaṣāye pāda-śeṣite ।
tailāḍhakaṃ sama-kṣīraṃ pacet kalkaiḥ palonmitaiḥ ।।

sthirā-tāmalakī-dūrvā-payasyābhīru-candanaiḥ ।
loha-haṃsapadī-māṃsī-dvi-medā-madhuparṇibhiḥ ।।

kākolī-kṣīra-kākolī-śatapuṣparddhi-padmakaiḥ ।
jīvakarṣabha-jīvantī-tvak-pattra-nakha-vālakaiḥ ।।

prapauṇḍarīka-mañjiṣṭhā-śārivaindrī-vitunnakaiḥ ।
catuṣ-prayogaṃ vātāsṛk-pitta-dāha-jvarārti-nut ।।

atuṣ-prayogāt tad dhanti ailaṃ māruta-śoṇitam
sopadravaṃ sāṅga-śūlaṃ sarva-gātrānugaṃ tathā ।
vātāsṛk-pitta-dāhārti-jvara-ghnaṃ bala-varṇa-kṛt ।।

balā-kaṣāya-kalkābhyāṃ tailaṃ kṣīra-samaṃ pacet ।
sahasra-śata-pākaṃ tad vātāsṛg-vāta-roga-nut ।।

rasāyanaṃ mukhya-tamam indriyāṇāṃ prasādanam ।
jīvanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ svaryaṃ śukrāsṛg-doṣa-nāśanam ।।

kupite mārga-saṃrodhān medaso vā kaphasya vā ।
ati-vṛddhyānile śastaṃ nādau snehana-bṛṃhaṇam ।।

kṛtvā tatrāḍhya-vātoktaṃ vāta-śoṇitikaṃ tataḥ ।
bheṣajaṃ snehanaṃ kuryād yac ca rakta-prasādanam ।।

prāṇādi-kope yuga-pad yathoddiṣṭaṃ yathāmayam ।
yathāsannaṃ ca bhaiṣajyaṃ vikalpyaṃ syād yathā-balam ।।

nīte nir-āma-tāṃ sāme sveda-laṅghana-pācanaiḥ ।
rūkṣaiś cālepa-sekādyaiḥ kuryāt kevala-vāta-nut ।।

śoṣākṣepaṇa-saṃkoca-stambha-svapana-kampanam ।
hanu-sraṃso arditaṃ khāñjyaṃ pāṅgulyaṃ khuḍa-vāta-tā ।।

saṃdhi-cyutiḥ pakṣa-vadho medo-majjāsthi-gā gadāḥ ।
ete sthānasya gāmbhīryāt sidhyeyur yatnato navāḥ ।।

tasmāj jayen navān etān balino nir-upadravān ।
vāyau pittāvṛte śītām uṣṇāṃ ca bahu-śaḥ kriyām ।।

vyatyāsād yojayet sarpir jīvanīyaṃ ca pāyayet ।
dhanva-māṃsaṃ yavāḥ śālir virekaḥ kṣīra-vān mṛduḥ ।।

sa-kṣīrā vastayaḥ kṣīraṃ pañca-mūla-balā-śṛtam ।
kāle anuvāsanaṃ tailair madhurauṣadha-sādhitaiḥ ।।

āle anuvāsanaṃ tailaṃ adhurauṣadha-sādhitam
yaṣṭīmadhu-balā-taila-ghṛta-kṣīraiś ca secanam ।
pañca-mūla-kaṣāyeṇa vāriṇā śītalena vā ।।

āriṇā śītalena ca
kaphāvṛte yavānnāni jāṅgalā mṛga-pakṣiṇaḥ ।
svedās tīkṣṇā nirūhāś ca vamanaṃ sa-virecanam ।।

purāṇa-sarpis tailaṃ ca tila-sarṣapa-jaṃ hitam ।
saṃsṛṣṭe kapha-pittābhyāṃ pittam ādau vinirjayet ।।

kārayed rakta-saṃsṛṣṭe vāta-śoṇitikīṃ kriyām ।
svedābhyaṅga-rasāḥ kṣīraṃ sneho māṃsāvṛte hitam ।।

neho māṃsāvṛte hitaḥ
prameha-medo-vāta-ghnam āḍhya-vāte bhiṣag-jitam ।
mahā-sneho asthi-majja-sthe pūrvoktaṃ retasāvṛte ।।

annāvṛte pācanīyaṃ vamanaṃ dīpanaṃ laghu ।
mūtrāvṛte mūtralāni svedāś cottara-vastayaḥ ।।

vedā uttara-vastayaḥ
eraṇḍa-tailaṃ varcaḥ-sthe vasti-snehāś ca bhedinaḥ ।
kapha-pittā-viruddhaṃ yad yac ca vātānulomanam ।।

sarva-sthānāvṛte apy āśu tat kāryaṃ mātariśvani ।
an-abhiṣyandi ca snigdhaṃ srotasāṃ śuddhi-kāraṇam ।।

arva-sthānāvṛte cāśu arva-sthānāvṛte tv āśu
yāpanā vastayaḥ prāyo madhurāḥ sānuvāsanāḥ ।
prasamīkṣya balādhikyaṃ mṛdu kāryaṃ virecanam ।।

ṛdu kāya-virecanam
rasāyanānāṃ sarveṣām upayogaḥ praśasyate ।
śilāhvasya viśeṣeṇa payasā śuddha-gugguloḥ ।।

leho vā bhārgavas tad-vad ekā-daśa-sitāśitaḥ ।
apāne tv āvṛte sarvaṃ dīpanaṃ grāhi bheṣajam ।।

kā-daśa-sitāsitaḥ
vātānulomanaṃ kāryaṃ mūtrāśaya-viśodhanam ।
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktam āvṛtānāṃ cikitsitam ।।

prāṇādīnāṃ bhiṣak kuryād vitarkya svayam eva tat ।
udānaṃ yojayed ūrdhvam apānaṃ cānulomayet ।।

samānaṃ śamayed vidvāṃs tri-dhā vyānaṃ tu yojayet ।
prāṇo rakṣyaś caturbhyo api tat-sthitau deha-saṃsthitiḥ ।।

ri-dhā vyānaṃ ca yojayet
svaṃ svaṃ sthānaṃ nayed evaṃ vṛtān vātān vi-mārga-gān ।
sarvaṃ cāvaraṇam pitta-rakta-saṃsarga-varjitam ।।

rasāyana-vidhānena laśuno hanti śīlitaḥ ।
pittāvṛte pitta-haraṃ marutaś cānulomanam ।।

raktāvṛte api tad-vac ca khuḍoktaṃ yac ca bheṣajam ।
rakta-pittānila-haraṃ vividhaṃ ca rasāyanam ।।

yathā-nidānaṃ nirdiṣṭam iti samyak cikitsitam ।
āyur-veda-phalaṃ sthānam etat sadyo arti-nāśanāt ।।

tat sadyo arti-nāśanam
cikitsitaṃ hitaṃ pathyaṃ prāyaścittaṃ bhiṣag-jitam ।
bheṣajaṃ śamanaṃ śastaṃ paryāyaiḥ smṛtam auṣadham ।।

kalpasthāna
vamane madanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ trivṛn-mūlaṃ virecane ।
nityam anyasya tu vyādhi-viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭa-tā ।।

phalāni nāti-pāṇḍūni na cāti-haritāny api ।
ādāyāhni praśatarkṣe madhye grīṣma-vasantayoḥ ।।

halāni tāni pāṇḍūni a cāti-haritāni ca a cāti-haritāny 
atha
pramṛjya kuśa-muttolyāṃ kṣiptvā baddhvā pralepayet ।
go-mayenānu muttolīṃ dhānya-madhye nidhāpayet ।।

ramṛjya kuśa-pūtolyāṃ o-mayenānu pūtolīṃ
mṛdu-bhūtāni madhv-iṣṭa-gandhāni kuśa-veṣṭanāt ।
niṣkṛṣṭāni gate aṣṭāhe śoṣayet tāny athātape ।।

ṛdu-bhūtāni madyeṣṭa- iṣkṛṣṭāni gatāṣṭāhe iṣkṛṣya nirgate aṣṭāhe 
iṣkṛṣya vigate aṣṭāhe
teṣāṃ tataḥ su-śuṣkāṇām uddhṛtya phala-pippalīḥ ।
dadhi-madhv-ājya-palalair mṛditvā śoṣayet punaḥ ।।

adhi-madhv-āmbu-palalair
tataḥ su-guptaṃ saṃsthāpya kārya-kāle prayojayet ।
athādāya tato mātrāṃ jarjarī-kṛtya vāsayet ।।

śarvarīṃ madhuyaṣṭyā vā kovidārasya vā jale ।
karbudārasya bimbyā vā nīpasya vidulasya vā ।।

īmūtakasya bimbyā vā
śaṇapuṣpyāḥ sadāpuṣpyāḥ pratyakpuṣpy-udake atha-vā ।
tataḥ pibet kaṣāyaṃ taṃ prātar mṛdita-gālitam ।।

ratyakpuṣpodake atha-vā ratyakpuṣpodakena vā
sūtroditena vidhinā sādhu tena tathā vamet ।
śleṣma-jvara-pratiśyāya-gulmāntar-vidradhīṣu ca ।।

ādhu tena yathā vamet ādhu tena tato vamet
pracchardayed viśeṣeṇa yāvat pittasya darśanam ।
phala-pippalī-cūrṇaṃ vā kvāthena svena bhāvitam ।।

tri-bhāga-tri-phalā-cūrṇaṃ kovidārādi-vāriṇā ।
pibej jvarā-ruci-ṣṭheva-granthy-apacy-arbudodarī ।।

ibej jvara-gara-ṣṭhīva- ibej jvara-gara-ṣṭheva- ibej jvara-gara-sveda- ibej jvarā-ruci-ṣṭhīva- ibej jvarā-ruciṣv evaṃ 
granthy-apacy-arbudodarī
pitte kapha-sthāna-gate jīmūtādi-jalena tat ।
hṛd-dāhe adho-'sra-pitte ca kṣīraṃ tat-pippalī-śṛtam ।।

kṣaireyīṃ vā kapha-cchardi-praseka-tamakeṣu tu ।
dadhy-uttaraṃ vā dadhi vā tac-chṛta-kṣīra-saṃbhavam ।।

-praseka-tamakeṣu ca
phalādi-kvātha-kalkābhyāṃ siddhaṃ tat-siddha-dugdha-jam ।
sarpiḥ kaphābhibhūte agnau śuṣyad-dehe ca vāmanam ।।

śuṣka-dehe ca vāmanam śuṣyad-dehe tu vāmanam
sva-rasaṃ phala-majjño vā bhallātaka-vidhi-śṛtam ।
ā-darvī-lepanāt siddhaṃ līḍhvā pracchardayet sukham ।।

taṃ lehaṃ bhakṣya-bhojyeṣu tat-kaṣāyāṃś ca yojayet ।
vatsakādi-pratīvāpaḥ kaṣāyaḥ phala-majja-jaḥ ।।

nimbārkānya-tara-kvātha-samāyukto niyacchati ।
baddha-mūlān api vyādhīn sarvān saṃtarpaṇodbhavān ।।

śleṣma-saṃtarpaṇodbhavān
rāṭha-puṣpa-phala-ślakṣṇa-cūrṇair mālyaṃ su-rūkṣitam ।
vamen maṇḍa-rasādīnāṃ tṛpto jighran sukhaṃ sukhī ।।

-cūrṇair mālyaṃ virūkṣitam -cūrṇair mālyaṃ su-rūṣitam -cūrṇair mālāṃ su-rūṣitām 
amen naro rasādīnāṃ
evam eva phalā-bhāve kalpyaṃ puṣpaṃ śalāṭu vā ।
jīmūtādyāś ca phala-vaj jīmūtaṃ tu viśeṣataḥ ।।

vam eva phalā-lābhe
prayoktavyaṃ jvara-śvāsa-kāsa-hidhmādi-rogiṇām ।
payaḥ puṣpe asya nirvṛtte phale peyā payas-kṛtā ।।

romaśe kṣīra-saṃtānaṃ dadhy-uttaram a-romaśe ।
śṛte payasi dadhy-amlaṃ jātaṃ harita-pāṇḍuke ।।

āte harita-pāṇḍuke āte harita-pāṇḍure ātaṃ 
harita-pāṇḍure
āsutya vāruṇī-maṇḍaṃ piben mṛdita-gālitam ।
kaphād a-rocake kāse pāṇḍu-tve rāja-yakṣmaṇi ।।

iyaṃ ca kalpanā kāryā tumbī-kośātakīṣv api ।
paryāgatānāṃ śuṣkāṇāṃ phalānāṃ veṇi-janmanām ।।

halānāṃ veṇu-janmanām halānāṃ coṇi-janmanām
cūrṇasya payasā śuktiṃ vāta-pittārditaḥ pibet ।
dve vā trīṇy api vāpothya kvāthe tiktottamasya vā ।।

ve vā trīṇy atha-vāpothya
āragvadhādi-navakād āsutyānya-tamasya vā ।
vimṛdya pūtaṃ taṃ kvāthaṃ pitta-śleṣma-jvarī pibet ।।

imṛjya pūtaṃ taṃ kvāthaṃ
jīmūta-kalkaṃ cūrṇaṃ vā pibec chītena vāriṇā ।
jvare paitte kavoṣṇena kapha-vātāt kaphād api ।।

īmūta-cūrṇaṃ kalkaṃ vā
kāsa-śvāsa-viṣa-cchardi-jvarārte kapha-karśite ।
ikṣvākur vamane śastaḥ pratāmyati ca mānave ।।

-jvarārte kapha-karṣite kṣvākur vamane śreṣṭhaḥ
phala-puṣpa-vihīnasya pravālais tasya sādhitam ।
pitta-śleṣma-jvare kṣīraṃ pittodrikte prayojayet ।।

ravālais tena sādhitam ittodreke prayojayet
hṛta-madhye phale jīrṇe sthitaṃ kṣīraṃ yadā dadhi ।
syāt tadā kapha-je kāse śvāse vamyaṃ ca pāyayet ।।

ṛta-madhye phale pakve śvāse vamyāṃ ca pāyayet
mastunā vā phalān madhyaṃ pāṇḍu-kuṣṭha-viṣārditaḥ ।
tena takraṃ vipakvaṃ vā pibet sa-madhu-saindhavam ।।

āṇduḥ kuṣṭhī viṣārditaḥ
bhāvayitvāja-dugdhena bījaṃ tenaiva vā pibet ।
viṣa-gulmodara-granthi-gaṇḍeṣu ślīpadeṣu ca ।।

saktubhir vā piben manthaṃ tumbī-sva-rasa-bhāvitaiḥ ।
kaphodbhave jvare kāse gala-rogeṣv a-rocake ।।

gulme jvare prasakte ca kalkaṃ māṃsa-rasaiḥ pibet ।
naraḥ sādhu vamaty evaṃ na ca daurbalyam aśnute ।।

ulme jvare praseke ca
tumbyāḥ phala-rasaiḥ śuṣkaiḥ sa-puṣpair avacūrṇitam ।
chardayen mālyam āghrāya gandha-saṃpat-sukhocitaḥ ।।

umbyāḥ phala-rasaiḥ śuṣkaṃ andhaṃ samyak sukhocitaḥ andha-saṃpat-sukhocitam 
andhaṃ samyak sukhocitam
kāsa-gulmodara-gare vāte śleṣmāśaya-sthite ।
kaphe ca kaṇṭha-vaktra-sthe kapha-saṃcaya-jeṣu ca ।।

apha-saṃcaya-jeṣu tu
dhāmārgavo gadeṣv iṣṭaḥ sthireṣu ca mahatsu ca ।
jīvakarṣabhakau vīrā kapikacchūḥ śatāvarī ।।

kākolī śrāvaṇī medā mahāmedā madhūlikā ।
tad-rajobhiḥ pṛthag lehā dhāmārgava-rajo-'nvitāḥ ।।

kāse hṛdaya-dāhe ca śastā madhu-sitā-drutāḥ ।
te sukhāmbho-'nu-pānāḥ syuḥ pittoṣma-sahite kaphe ।।

śastā madhu-sitā-yutāḥ śastā madhu-sitānvitāḥ
dhānya-tumburu-yūṣeṇa kalkas tasya viṣāpahaḥ ।
bimbyāḥ punarnavāyā vā kāsamardasya vā rase ।।

imbyāḥ punarnavāyāś ca
ekaṃ dhāmārgavaṃ dve vā mānase mṛditaṃ pibet ।
tac-chṛta-kṣīra-jaṃ sarpiḥ sādhitaṃ vā phalādibhiḥ ।।

kṣveḍo ati-kaṭu-tīkṣṇoṣṇaḥ pragāḍheṣu praśasyate ।
kuṣṭha-pāṇḍv-āmaya-plīha-śopha-gulma-garādiṣu ।।

ragāḍheṣu ca śasyate
pṛthak phalādi-ṣaṭkasya kvāthe māṃsam anūpa-jam ।
kośātakyā samaṃ siddhaṃ tad-rasaṃ lavaṇaṃ pibet ।।

ośātakyāḥ samaṃ siddhaṃ
phalādi-pippalī-tulyaṃ siddhaṃ kṣveḍa-rase atha-vā ।
kṣveḍa-kvāthaṃ pibet siddhaṃ miśram ikṣu-rasena vā ।।

iddhaṃ kṣveḍa-rasena vā ṣveḍa-kvāthe pibet siddhaṃ
kauṭajaṃ su-kumāreṣu pitta-rakta-kaphodaye ।
jvare visarpe hṛd-roge khuḍe kuṣṭhe ca pūjitam ।।

uṭajaṃ su-kumāreṣu
sarṣapāṇāṃ madhūkānāṃ toyena lavaṇasya vā ।
pāyayet kauṭajaṃ bījaṃ yuktaṃ kṛśarayātha-vā ।।

saptāhaṃ vārka-dugdhāktaṃ tac-cūrṇaṃ pāyayet pṛthak ।
phala-jīmūtakekṣvāku-jīvantī-jīvakodakaiḥ ।।

aptāhaṃ cārka-dughāktaṃ
vamanauṣadha-mukhyānām iti kalpa-dig īritā ।
bījenānena mati-mān anyāny api ca kalpayet ।।

idhinānena mati-mān nyān api ca kalpayet nyān api ca yojayet

kalpasthāna
kaṣāya-madhurā rūkṣā vipāke kaṭukā trivṛt ।
kapha-pitta-praśamanī raukṣyāc cānila-kopanī ।।

aṣāyā madhurā rūkṣā aukṣyāt sānila-kopanī aukṣyād 
anila-kopanī
sedānīm auṣadhair yuktā vāta-pitta-kaphāpahaiḥ ।
kalpa-vaiśeṣyam āsādya jāyate sarva-roga-jit ।।

dvi-dhā khyātaṃ ca tan-mūlaṃ śyāmaṃ śyāmāruṇaṃ trivṛt ।
trivṛd-ākhyaṃ vara-taraṃ nir-apāyaṃ sukhaṃ tayoḥ ।।

su-kumāre śiśau vṛddhe mṛdu-koṣṭhe ca tad dhitam ।
mūrchā-saṃmoha-hṛt-kaṇṭha-kaṣaṇa-kṣaṇana-pradam ।।

-karṣaṇa-kṣaṇana-pradam
śyāmaṃ tīkṣṇāśu-kāri-tvād atas tad api śasyate ।
krūre koṣṭhe bahau doṣe kleśa-kṣamiṇi cāture ।।

rūre koṣṭhe bahu-doṣe rūre koṣṭhe mahā-doṣe
gambhīrānugataṃ ślakṣṇam a-tiryag-visṛtaṃ ca yat ।
gṛhītvā visṛjet kāṣṭhaṃ tvacaṃ śuṣkāṃ nidhāpayet ।।

-tiryag-vistṛtaṃ ca yat
atha kāle tataś cūrṇaṃ kiñ-cin nāgara-saindhavam ।
vātāmaye pibed amlaiḥ paitte sājya-sitā-madhu ।।

tha kāle ca tac-cūrṇaṃ tha kāle tu tac-cūrṇaṃ tha kāle trivṛc-cūrṇaṃ tha kālena tac-cūrṇaṃ ātāmayī pibed amlaiḥ itte 
sājya-sitā-madhu
kṣīra-drākṣekṣu-kāśmarya-svādu-skandha-varā-rasaiḥ ।
kaphāmaye pīlu-rasa-mūtra-madyāmla-kāñjikaiḥ ।।

pañca-kolādi-cūrṇaiś ca yuktyā yuktaṃ kaphāpahaiḥ ।
trivṛt-kalka-kaṣāyābhyāṃ sādhitaḥ sa-sito himaḥ ।।

rivṛt-kalka-kaṣāyeṇa uktaṃ yuñjyāt kaphāpahaiḥ
madhu-tri-jāta-saṃyukto leho hṛdyaṃ virecanam ।
ajagandhā tavakṣīrī vidārī śarkarā trivṛt ।।

jagandhā tukākṣīrī
cūrṇitaṃ madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ līḍhvā sādhu viricyate ।
saṃnipāta-jvara-stambha-pipāsā-dāha-pīḍitaḥ ।।

ac-cūrṇaṃ madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ
limped antas trivṛtayā dvi-dhā kṛtvekṣu-gaṇḍikām ।
ekī-kṛtya ca tat svinnaṃ puṭa-pākena bhakṣayet ।।

vi-dhā kṛtvekṣu-gaṇḍikāḥ vi-dhā kṛtvekṣu-kaṇḍikām vi-dhā kṛtvekṣu-kāṇḍikām kī-kṛtaṃ ca tat svinnaṃ kī-kṛtya ca su-svinnaṃ 
ekī-kṛtya tu tat svinnaṃ
bhṛṅgailābhyāṃ samā nīlī tais trivṛtaiś ca śarkarā ।
cūrṇaṃ phala-rasa-kṣaudra-saktubhis tarpaṇaṃ pibet ।।

vag-elābhyāṃ samā nīlī
vāta-pitta-kaphottheṣu rogeṣv alpānaleṣu ca ।
nareṣu su-kumāreṣu nir-apāyaṃ virecanam ।।

viḍaṅga-taṇḍula-varā-yāva-śūka-kaṇās trivṛt ।
sarvato ardhena tal līḍhaṃ madhv-ājyena guḍena vā ।।

gulmaṃ plīhodaraṃ kāsaṃ halīmakam a-rocakam ।
kapha-vāta-kṛtāṃś cānyān parimārṣṭi gadān bahūn ।।

viḍaṅga-pippalī-mūla-tri-phalā-dhānya-citrakān ।
marīcendrayavājājī-pippalī-hasti-pippalīḥ ।।

-tri-phalā-dhānya-citrakam -pippalī-hasti-pippali
dīpyakaṃ pañca-lavaṇaṃ cūrṇitaṃ kārṣikaṃ pṛthak ।
tila-taila-trivṛc-cūrṇa-bhāgau cāṣṭa-palonmitau ।।

-bhāgāv aṣṭa-palonmitau
dhātrī-phala-rasa-prasthāṃs trīn guḍārdha-tulānvitān ।
paktvā mṛdv-agninā khādet tato mātrām a-yantraṇaḥ ।।

rīn guḍārdha-tulonmitān ato mātrām a-yantritaḥ mandāgni-tvaṃ jvaraṃ mūrchāṃ mūtra-kṛcchram a-rocakam ।।

kuṣṭhārśaḥ-kāmalā-gulma-mehodara-bhagandarān ।
grahaṇī-pāṇḍu-rogāṃś ca hanti puṃ-savanaś ca saḥ ।।

guḍaḥ kalyāṇako nāma sarveṣv ṛtuṣu yaugikaḥ ।
vyoṣa-tri-jātakāmbhoda-kṛmighnāmalakais trivṛt ।।

sarvaiḥ samā sama-sitā kṣaudreṇa guṭikāḥ kṛtāḥ ।
mūtra-kṛcchra-jvara-cchardi-kāsa-śoṣa-bhrama-kṣaye ।।

arvaiḥ samānā sa-sitā ṣaudreṇa guṭikī-kṛtā bhakṣayet prātar utthāya śītaṃ cānu pibej jalam ।।

tāpe pāṇḍv-āmaye alpe agnau śastāḥ sarva-viṣeṣu ca ।
a-vipattir ayaṃ yogaḥ praśastaḥ pitta-rogiṇām ।।

trivṛtā kauṭajaṃ bījaṃ pippalī viśva-bheṣajam ।
kṣaudra-drākṣā-rasopetaṃ varṣā-kāle virecanam ।।

trivṛd-durālabhā-musta-śarkarodīcya-candanam ।
drākṣāmbunā sa-yaṣṭy-āhva-sātalaṃ jala-dātyaye ।।

rākṣāmbunā sa-yaṣṭy-āhvaṃ -śītalaṃ jala-dātyaye 
śītalaṃ jala-dātyaye
trivṛtāṃ citrakaṃ pāṭhām ajājīṃ saralaṃ vacām ।
svarṇakṣīrīṃ ca hemante cūrṇam uṣṇāmbunā pibet ।।

trivṛtā śarkarā-tulyā grīṣma-kāle virecanam ।
trivṛt-trāyanti-hapuṣā-sātalā-kaṭu-rohiṇīḥ ।।

svarṇakṣīrīṃ ca saṃcūrṇya go-mūtre bhāvayet try-aham ।
eṣa sarvartuko yogaḥ snigdhānāṃ mala-doṣa-hṛt ।।

śyāmā-trivṛd-durālabhā-hasti-pippalī-vatsakam ।
nīlinī-kaṭukā-mustā-śreṣṭhā-yuktaṃ su-cūrṇitam ।।

rasājyoṣṇāmbubhiḥ śastaṃ rūkṣāṇām api sarva-dā ।
jvara-hṛd-roga-vātāsṛg-udāvartādi-rogiṣu ।।

saindhavaṃ pippalī-mūlam abhayā dvi-guṇottaram ।
cūrṇam uṣṇāmbunā peyaṃ svasthe sukha-virecanam ।।

ūrṇam uṣṇāmbunā pītaṃ
rājavṛkṣo adhikaṃ pathyo mṛdur madhura-śītalaḥ ।
bāle vṛddhe kṣate kṣīṇe su-kumāre ca mānave ।।

yojyo mṛdv-an-apāyi-tvād viśeṣāc caturaṅgulaḥ ।
phala-kāle pariṇataṃ phalaṃ tasya samāharet ।।

teṣāṃ guṇa-vatāṃ bhāraṃ sikatāsu vinikṣipet ।
sapta-rātrāt samuddhṛtya śoṣayed ātape tataḥ ।।

śoṣayec cātape tataḥ śoṣayed ātape punaḥ
tato majjānam uddhṛtya śucau pātre nidhāpayet ।
drākṣā-rasena taṃ dadyād dāhodāvarta-pīḍite ।।

catur-varṣe sukhaṃ bāle yāvad dvā-daśa-vārṣike ।
caturaṅgula-majjño vā kaṣāyaṃ pāyayed dhimam ।।

dadhi-maṇḍa-surā-maṇḍa-dhātrī-phala-rasaiḥ pṛthak ।
sauvīrakeṇa vā yuktaṃ kalkena traivṛtena vā ।।

dantī-kaṣāye tan-majjño guḍaṃ jīrṇaṃ ca nikṣipet ।
tam ariṣṭaṃ sthitaṃ māsaṃ pāyayet pakṣam eva vā ।।

tvacaṃ tilvaka-mūlasya tyaktvābhyantara-valkalam ।
viśoṣya cūrṇayitvā ca dvau bhāgau gālayet tataḥ ।।

lodhrasyaiva kaṣāyeṇa tṛtīyaṃ tena bhāvayet ।
kaṣāye daśa-mūlasya taṃ bhāgaṃ bhāvitaṃ punaḥ ।।

odhrasya tu kaṣāyeṇa
śuṣkaṃ cūrṇaṃ punaḥ kṛtvā tataḥ pāṇi-talaṃ pibet ।
mastu-mūtra-surā-maṇḍa-kola-dhātrī-phalāmbubhiḥ ।।

śuṣka-cūrṇaṃ tataḥ kuryāt śuṣka-cūrṇaṃ punaḥ kṛtvā 
śuṣkaṃ cūrṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā
tilvakasya kaṣāyeṇa kalkena ca sa-śarkaraḥ ।
sa-ghṛtaḥ sādhito lehaḥ sa ca śreṣṭhaṃ virecanam ।।

a ca śreṣṭho virecanam
sudhā bhinatti doṣāṇāṃ mahāntam api saṃcayam ।
āśv eva kaṣṭa-vibhraṃśān naiva tāṃ kalpayed ataḥ ।।

āśv eva kaṣṭa-vibhraṃśāṃ āśv eva koṣṭha-vibhraṃśān 
naiva tāṃ kalpayet tataḥ
mṛdau koṣṭhe a-bale bāle sthavire dīrgha-rogiṇi ।
kalpyā gulmodara-gara-tvag-roga-madhu-mehiṣu ।।

pāṇḍau dūṣī-viṣe śophe doṣa-vibhrānta-cetasi ।
sā śreṣṭhā kaṇṭakais tīkṣṇair bahubhiś ca samācitā ।।

dvi-varṣāṃ vā tri-varṣāṃ vā śiśirānte viśeṣataḥ ।
tāṃ pāṭayitvā śastreṇa kṣīram uddhārayet tataḥ ।।

bilvādīnāṃ bṛhatyor vā kvāthena samam eka-śaḥ ।
miśrayitvā sudhā-kṣīraṃ tato aṅgāreṣu śoṣayet ।।

pibet kṛtvā tu guṭikāṃ mastu-mūtra-surādibhiḥ ।
trivṛtādīn nava varāṃ svarṇakṣīrīṃ sa-sātalām ।।

saptāhaṃ snuk-payaḥ-pītān rasenājyena vā pibet ।
tad-vad vyoṣottamā-kumbha-nikumbhāgnīn guḍāmbunā ।।

-nikumbhādīn guḍāmbunā
nāti-śuṣkaṃ phalaṃ grāhyaṃ śaṅkhinyā nis-tuṣī-kṛtam ।
saptalāyās tathā mūlaṃ te tu tīkṣṇa-vikāṣiṇī ।।

śleṣmāmayodara-gara-śvayathv-ādiṣu kalpayet ।
akṣa-mātraṃ tayoḥ piṇḍaṃ madirā-lavaṇānvitam ।।

hṛd-roge vāta-kapha-je tad-vad gulme api yojayet ।
danti-danta-sthiraṃ sthūlaṃ mūlaṃ dantī-dravanti-jam ।।

ad-vad gulme prayojay et
ā-tāmra-śyāva-tīkṣṇoṣṇam āśu-kāri vikāśi ca ।
guru prakopi vātasya pitta-śleṣma-vilāyanam ।।

āśu-kāri vikāṣi ca
tat kṣaudra-pippalī-liptaṃ svedyaṃ mṛd-darbha-veṣṭitam ।
śoṣyaṃ mandātape agny-arkau hato hy asya vikāśi-tām ।।

at kṣaudra-pippalī-miśraṃ at kṣaudra-pippalī-yuktaṃ 
hato hy asya vikāṣi-tām
tat piben mastu-madirā-takra-pīlu-rasāsavaiḥ ।
abhiṣyaṇṇa-tanur gulmī pramehī jaṭharī garī ।।

bhiṣyanda-tanur gulmī bhiṣyandi-tanur gulmī
go-mṛgāja-rasaiḥ pāṇḍuḥ kṛmi-koṣṭhī bhagandarī ।
siddhaṃ tat kvātha-kalkābhyāṃ daśa-mūla-rasena ca ।।

visarpa-vidradhy-alajī-kakṣā-dāhān jayed ghṛtam ।
tailaṃ tu gulma-mehārśo-vibandha-kapha-mārutān ।।

mahā-snehaḥ śakṛc-chukra-vāta-saṅgānila-vyathāḥ ।
virecane mukhya-tamā navaite trivṛtādayaḥ ।।

ahā-snehaś ca viṭ-śukra-
harītakīm api trivṛd-vidhānenopakalpayet ।
guḍasyāṣṭa-pale pathyā viṃśatiḥ syāt palaṃ palam ।।

dantī-citrakayoḥ karṣau pippalī-trivṛtor daśa ।
prakalpya modakān ekaṃ daśame daśame ahani ।।

uṣṇāmbho anupibet khādet tān sarvān vidhināmunā ।
ete niṣ-parihārāḥ syuḥ sarva-vyādhi-nibarhaṇāḥ ।।

ṣṇāmbho anupiban khādet
viśeṣād grahaṇī-pāṇḍu-kaṇḍū-koṭhārśasāṃ hitāḥ ।
alpasyāpi mahārtha-tvaṃ prabhūtasyālpa-karma-tām ।।

-kaṇḍū-koṣṭhāṛśasāṃ hitāḥ -kaṇḍū-kuṣṭhāṛśasāṃ hitāḥ kuryāt saṃśleṣa-viśleṣa-kāla-saṃskāra-yuktibhiḥ ।।

ū̆-kāla-saṃskāra-yuktitaḥ
tvak-kesarāmrātaka-dāḍimailā-sitopalā-mākṣika-mātuluṅgaiḥ ।
madyena tais taiś ca mano-'nukūlair yuktāni deyāni virecanāni ।।

adyaiś ca tais taiś ca mano-'nukūlair

kalpasthāna
vamanaṃ mṛdu-koṣṭhena kṣud-vatālpa-kaphena vā ।
ati-tīkṣṇa-hima-stokam a-jīrṇe dur-balena vā ।।

pītaṃ prayāty adhas tasminn iṣṭa-hānir malodayaḥ ।
vāmayet taṃ punaḥ snigdhaṃ smaran pūrvam atikramam ।।

maran pūrvam anu-kramam
a-jīrṇinaḥ śleṣma-vato vrajaty ūrdhvaṃ virecanam ।
ati-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-lavaṇam a-hṛdyam ati-bhūri vā ।।

tatra pūrvoditā vyāpat siddhiś ca na tathāpi cet ।
āśaye tiṣṭhati tatas tṛtīyaṃ nāvacārayet ।।

anya-tra sātmyād dhṛdyād vā bheṣajān nir-apāyataḥ ।
a-snigdha-svinna-dehasya purāṇaṃ rūkṣam auṣadham ।।

nya-tra sātmyād dhṛdyād ca -snigdhā-svinna-dehasya
doṣān utkleśya nirhartum a-śaktaṃ janayed gadān ।
vibhraṃśaṃ śvayathuṃ hidhmāṃ tamaso darśanaṃ tṛṣam ।।

id-bhraṃśaṃ śvayathuṃ hidhmāṃ
piṇḍikodveṣṭanaṃ kaṇḍūm ūrvoḥ sādaṃ vi-varṇa-tām ।
snigdha-svinnasya vāty-alpaṃ dīptāgner jīrṇam auṣadham ।।

nigdha-svinnasya cāty-alpaṃ
śītair vā stabdham āme vā samutkleśyāharan malān ।
tān eva janayed rogān a-yogaḥ sarva eva saḥ ।।

śītair vā stabdham āmair vā amutkleśyāharen malān 
samutkleśya haren malān
taṃ taila-lavaṇābhyaktaṃ svinnaṃ prastara-saṃkaraiḥ ।
nirūḍhaḥ jāṅgala-rasair bhojayitvānuvāsayet ।।

vinnaṃ saṃstara-saṃkaraiḥ vinnaṃ saṃstara-śaṅkaraiḥ
phala-māgadhikā-dāru-siddha-tailena mātrayā ।
snigdhaṃ vāta-haraiḥ snehaiḥ punas tīkṣṇena śodhayet ।।

bahu-doṣasya rūkṣasya mandāgner alpam auṣadham ।
sodāvartasya cotkleśya doṣān mārgān nirudhya taiḥ ।।

oṣān mārgaṃ nirudhya taiḥ
bhṛśam ādhmāpayen nābhiṃ pṛṣṭha-pārśva-śiro-rujam ।
śvāsaṃ viṇ-mūtra-vātānāṃ saṅgaṃ kuryāc ca dāruṇam ।।

hṛśam ādhmāpayen nābhi- -pṛṣṭha-pārśva-śiro-rujam
abhyaṅga-sveda-varty-ādi sa-nirūhānuvāsanam ।
udāvarta-haram sarvaṃ karmādhmātasya śasyate ।।

pañca-mūla-yava-kṣāra-vacā-bhūtika-saindhavaiḥ ।
yavāgūḥ su-kṛtā śūla-vibandhānāha-nāśanī ।।

añca-kola-yava-kṣāra-
pippalī-dāḍima-kṣāra-hiṅgu-śuṇṭhy-amla-vetasān ।
sa-saindhavān piben madyaiḥ sarpiṣoṣṇodakena vā ।।

pravāhikā-parisrāva-vedanā-parikartane ।
pītauṣadhasya vegānāṃ nigrahān mārutādayaḥ ।।

ravāhikā-parisrāve edanā-parikartane
kupitā hṛdayaṃ gatvā ghoraṃ kurvanti hṛd-graham ।
hidhmā-pārśva-rujā-kāsa-dainya-lālākṣi-vibhramaiḥ ।।

jihvāṃ khādati niḥ-saṃjño dantān kaṭakaṭāyayan ।
na gacched vibhramaṃ tatra vāmayed āśu taṃ bhiṣak ।।

antān kaṭakaṭāyate
madhuraiḥ pitta-mūrchārtaṃ kaṭubhiḥ kapha-mūrchitam ।
pācanīyais tataś cāsya doṣa-śeṣaṃ vipācayet ।।

ācanīyais tataś cāśu oṣa-śeṣaṃ ca pācayet
kāyāgniṃ ca balaṃ cāsya krameṇābhipravardhayet ।
pavanenāti-vamato hṛdayaṃ yasya pīḍyate ।।

rameṇābhipravartayet
tasmai snigdhāmla-lavaṇān dadyāt pitta-kaphe anya-thā ।
pītauṣadhasya vegānāṃ nigraheṇa kaphena vā ।।

asmai snigdhāmla-lavaṇaṃ
ruddho ati vā viśuddhasya gṛhṇāty aṅgāni mārutaḥ ।
stambha-vepathu-nistoda-sādodveṣṭārti-bhedanaiḥ ।।

uddho vāti viśuddhasya -sādodveṣṭādhibhedanaiḥ
tatra vāta-haraṃ sarvaṃ sneha-svedādi śasyate ।
bahu-tīkṣṇaṃ kṣudhārtasya mṛdu-koṣṭhasya bheṣajam ।।

hṛtvāśu viṭ-pitta-kaphān dhātūn āsrāvayed dravān ।
tatrāti-yoge madhuraiḥ śeṣam auṣadham ullikhet ।।

hātūn prasrāvayed dravān
yojyo ati-vamane reko vireke vamanaṃ mṛdu ।
pariṣekāvagāhādyaiḥ su-śītaiḥ stambhayec ca tam ।।

ojyo ati reko vamite
añjanaṃ candanośīram ajāsṛk-śarkarodakam ।
lāja-cūrṇaiḥ piben mantham ati-yoga-haraṃ param ।।

ñjanaṃ candanośīra- -majjāsṛk-śarkarodakam
vamanasyāti-yoge tu śītāmbu-pariṣecitaḥ ।
pibet phala-rasair manthaṃ sa-ghṛta-kṣaudra-śarkaram ।।

sodgārāyāṃ bhṛśaṃ chardyāṃ mūrvāyā dhānya-mustayoḥ ।
sa-madhūkāñjanaṃ cūrṇaṃ lehayen madhu-saṃyutam ।।

ūrchāyāṃ dhānya-mustayoḥ
vamato antaḥ praviṣṭāyāṃ jihvāyāṃ kavaḍa-grahāḥ ।
snigdhāmla-lavaṇā hṛdyā yūṣa-māṃsa-rasā hitāḥ ।।

nigdhāmla-lavaṇā hṛdyāś hāga-māṃsa-rasā hitāḥ
phalāny amlāni khādeyus tasya cānye agrato narāḥ ।
niḥsṛtāṃ tu tila-drākṣā-kalka-liptāṃ praveśayet ।।

asya cānye agrato janāḥ asya caivāgrato narāḥ 
-kalka-liptāṃ prayojayet
vāg-grahānila-rogeṣu ghṛta-māṃsopasādhitām ।
yavāgūṃ tanukāṃ dadyāt sneha-svedau ca kāla-vit ।।

ati-yogāc ca bhaiṣajyaṃ jīvaṃ harati śoṇitam ।
taj jīvādānam ity uktam ādatte jīvitaṃ yataḥ ।।

ādhatte jīvanaṃ nṛṇām
śune kākāya vā dadyāt tenānnam asṛjā saha ।
bhukte a-bhukte vadej jīvaṃ pittaṃ vā bheṣajeritam ।।

huktā-bhuktaṃ vadej jīvaṃ hukte tasmin vadej jīvam huktvā-bhukte vadej jīvaṃ 
-bhukte pittam ādiśet
śuklaṃ vā bhāvitaṃ vastram āvānaṃ koṣṇa-vāriṇā ।
prakṣālitaṃ vi-varṇaṃ syāt pitte śuddhaṃ tu śoṇite ।।

ittaṃ śuddhaṃ tu śoṇitaṃ
tṛṣṇā-mūrchā-madārtasya kuryād ā-maraṇāt kriyām ।
rakta-pittātisāra-ghnīṃ tasyāśu prāṇa-rakṣaṇīm ।।

uryād ā-maraṇa-kriyām asyāpi prāṇa-rakṣaṇīm
mṛga-go-mahiṣājānāṃ sadyaskaṃ jīvatām asṛk ।
pibej jīvābhisaṃdhānaṃ jīvaṃ tad dhy āśu gacchati ।।

īvaṃ tad dhy āśu yacchati
tad eva darbha-mṛditaṃ raktaṃ vastau niṣecayet ।
śyāmā-kāśmarya-madhuka-dūrvośīraiḥ śṛtaṃ payaḥ ।।

ghṛta-maṇḍāñjana-yutaṃ vastiṃ vā yojayed dhimam ।
picchā-vastiṃ su-śītaṃ vā ghṛta-maṇḍānuvāsanam ।।

gudaṃ bhraṣṭaṃ kaṣāyaiś ca stambhayitvā praveśayet ।
vi-saṃjñaṃ śrāvayet sāma-veṇu-gītādi-nisvanam ।।

tambhayitvā prayojayet

kalpasthāna
balāṃ guḍūcīṃ tri-phalāṃ sa-rāsnāṃ dvi-pañca-mūlaṃ ca palonmitāni ।
aṣṭau phalāny ardha-tulāṃ ca māṃsāc chāgāt paced apsu caturtha-śeṣam ।।

pūto yavānī-phala-bilva-kuṣṭha-vacā-śatāhvā-ghana-pippalīnām ।
kalkair guḍa-kṣaudra-ghṛtaiḥ sa-tailair yuktaḥ sukhoṣṇo lavaṇānvitaś ca ।।

ūtaṃ yavānī-phala-bilva-kuṣṭha-
vastiḥ paraṃ sarva-gada-pramāthī svasthe hito jīvana-bṛṃhaṇaś ca ।
vastau ca yasmin paṭhito na kalkaḥ sarva-tra dadyād amum eva tatra ।।

astau ca yasmin kathito na kalkaḥ
dvi-pañca-mūlasya raso amla-yuktaḥ sa-cchāga-māṃsasya sa-pūrva-peṣyaḥ ।
tri-sneha-yuktaḥ pravaro nirūhaḥ sarvānila-vyādhi-haraḥ pradiṣṭaḥ ।।

a-cchāga-māṃsasya sa-pūrva-kalkaḥ
balā-paṭolī-laghu-pañca-mūla-trāyantikairaṇḍa-yavāt su-siddhāt ।
prastho rasāc chāga-rasārdha-yuktaḥ sādhyaḥ punaḥ prastha-samaḥ sa yāvat ।।

priyaṅgu-kṛṣṇā-ghana-kalka-yuktaḥ sa-taila-sarpir-madhu-saindhavaś ca ।
syād dīpano māṃsa-bala-pradaś ca cakṣur-balaṃ copadadhāti sadyaḥ ।।

eraṇḍa-mūlāt tri-palaṃ palāśāt tathā palāṃśaṃ laghu-pañca-mūlam ।
rāsnā-balā-chinnaruhāśvagandhā-punarnavāragvadha-devadāru ।।

athā palāṃśaṃ laghu-pañca-mūlāt
phalāni cāṣṭau salilāḍhakābhyāṃ vipācayed aṣṭama-śeṣite asmin ।
vacā-śatāhvā-hapuṣā-priyaṅgu-yaṣṭī-kaṇā-vatsaka-bīja-mustam ।।

dadyāt su-piṣṭaṃ saha-tārkṣya-śailam akṣa-pramāṇaṃ lavaṇāṃśa-yuktam ।
sa-mākṣikas taila-yutaḥ sa-mūtro vastir jayel lekhana-dīpano asau ।।

astir jayed dīpana-pācano asau
jaṅghoru-pāda-trika-pṛṣṭha-koṣṭha-hṛd-guhya-śūlaṃ guru-tāṃ vibandham ।
gulmāśma-vardhma-grahaṇī-gudotthāṃs tās tāṃś ca rogān kapha-vāta-jātān ।।

ulmāśma-vardhma-grahaṇī-vikārāṃs āṃs tāṃś ca rogān 
kapha-vāta-jāṃś ca
yaṣṭy-āhva-lodhrābhaya-candanaiś ca śṛtaṃ payo agryaṃ kamalotpalaiś ca ।
sa-śarkarā-kṣaudra-ghṛtaṃ su-śītaṃ pittāmayān hanti sa-jīvanīyam ।।

a-śarkaraṃ kṣaudra-yutaṃ su-śītaṃ ittāmayaṃ hanti 
sa-jīvanīyam
rāsnāṃ vṛṣaṃ lohitikām anantāṃ balāṃ kanīyas-tṛṇa-pañca-mūlyau ।
gopāṅganā-candana-padmakarddhi-yaṣṭy-āhva-lodhrāṇi palārdhakāni ।।

opāṅganā-candana-padmakāhva-
niḥkvāthya toyena rasena tena śṛtaṃ payo ardhāḍhakam ambu-hīnam ।
jīvanti-medarddhi-varī-vidārī-vīrā-dvi-kākoli-kaserukābhiḥ ।।

sitopalā-jīvaka-padma-reṇu-prapauṇḍarīkotpala-puṇḍarīkaiḥ ।
lodhrātmaguptā-madhuyaṣṭikābhir nāgāhva-muñjātaka-candanaiś ca ।।

ohātmaguptā-madhuyaṣṭikābhir
piṣṭair ghṛta-kṣaudra-yutair nirūhaṃ sa-saindhavaṃ śītalam eva dadyāt ।
pratyāgate dhanva-rasena śālīn kṣīreṇa vādyāt pariṣikta-gātraḥ ।।

dāhātisāra-pradarāsra-pitta-hṛt-pāṇḍu-rogān viṣama-jvaraṃ ca ।
sa-gulma-mūtra-graha-kāmalādīn sarvāmayān pitta-kṛtān nihanti ।।

āhātisāra-pradarāmla-pitta- -hṛt-pāṇḍu-rogān viṣama-jvarāṃś ca 
-hṛt-pāṇḍu-rogān viṣamān jvarāṃś ca
kośātakāragvadha-devadāru-mūrvā-śvadaṃṣṭrā-kuṭajārka-pāṭhāḥ ।
paktvā kulatthān bṛhatīṃ ca toye rasasya tasya prasṛtā daśa syuḥ ।।

tān sarṣapailā-madanaiḥ sa-kuṣṭhair akṣa-pramāṇaiḥ prasṛtaiś ca yuktān ।
kṣaudrasya tailasya phalāhvayasya kṣārasya tailasya ca sārṣapasya ।।

ṣārasya tailasya ca sarṣapasya
dadyān nirūhaṃ kapha-rogitāya mandāgnaye cāśana-vidviṣe ca ।
vakṣye mṛdūn sneha-kṛto nirūhān sukhocitānāṃ prasṛtaiḥ pṛthak tu ।।

athemān su-kumārāṇāṃ nirūhān snehanān mṛdūn ।
karmaṇā viplutānāṃ ca vakṣyāmi prasṛtaiḥ pṛthak ।।

armaṇā viplutānāṃ tu
kṣīrād dvau prasṛtau kāryau madhu-taila-ghṛtāt trayaḥ ।
khajena mathito vastir vāta-ghno bala-varṇa-kṛt ।।

ekaikaḥ prasṛtas taila-prasannā-kṣaudra-sarpiṣām ।
bilvādi-mūla-kvāthād dvau kaulatthād dvau sa vāta-jit ।।

kaikaḥ prasṛtis taila-
paṭola-nimba-bhūtīka-rāsnā-saptacchadāmbhasaḥ ।
prasṛtaḥ pṛthag ājyāc ca vastiḥ sarṣapa-kalka-vān ।।

aṭola-nimba-pūtīka- -rāsnā-saptacchadāmbhasām 
prasṛtāḥ pṛthag ājyāc ca
sa pañca-tikto abhiṣyanda-kṛmi-kuṣṭha-prameha-hā ।
catvāras taila-go-mūtra-dadhi-maṇḍāmla-kāñjikāt ।।

-kṛmi-kuṣṭha-pramoha-hā -kṛmi-kuṣṭha-prameha-jit
prasṛtāḥ sarṣapaiḥ piṣṭair viṭ-saṅgānāha-bhedanaḥ ।
payasyekṣu-sthirā-rāsnā-vidārī-kṣaudra-sarpiṣām ।।

iṭ-saṅgānāha-bhedanāḥ iṭ-saṅgānāha-bhedinaḥ 
-vidārī-kṣaudra-sarpiṣaḥ
ekaikaḥ prasṛto vastiḥ kṛṣṇā-kalko vṛṣa-tva-kṛt ।
siddha-vastīn ato vakṣye sarva-dā yān prayojayet ।।

nir-vyāpado bahu-phalān bala-puṣṭi-karān sukhān ।
madhu-taile same karṣaḥ saindhavād dvi-picur miśiḥ ।।

eraṇḍa-mūla-kvāthena nirūho mādhutailikaḥ ।
rasāyanaṃ pramehārśaḥ-kṛmi-gulmāntra-vṛddhi-nut ।।

irūho madhu-tailikaḥ -kṛmi-gulmāntra-vṛddhi-hṛt
sa-yaṣṭīmadhukaś caiṣa cakṣuṣyo rakta-pitta-jit ।
yāpano ghana-kalkena madhu-taila-rasājya-vān ।।

pāyu-jānūru-vṛṣaṇa-vasti-mehana-śūla-jit ।
prasṛtāṃśair ghṛta-kṣaudra-vasā-tailaiḥ prakalpayet ।।

āyu-jaṅghoru-vṛṣaṇa-
yāpanaṃ saindhavārdhākṣa-hapuṣārdha-palānvitam ।
eraṇḍa-mūla-niḥkvātho madhu-tailaṃ sa-saindhavam ।।

adhu-tailaṃ sa-saindhavaḥ
eṣa yukta-ratho vastiḥ sa-vacā-pillalī-phalaḥ ।
sa kvātho madhu-ṣaḍgranthā-śatāhvā-hiṅgu-saindhavam ।।

at-kvātho madhu-ṣaḍgranthā- -śatāhvā-hiṅgu-saindhavaḥ
suradāru ca rāsnā ca vastir doṣa-haraḥ śivaḥ ।
pañca-mūlasya niḥkvāthas tailaṃ māgadhikā madhu ।।

uradāru vacā rāsnā astir doṣa-haraś ca saḥ astir 
doṣa-haraḥ paraḥ
sa-saindhavaḥ sa-madhukaḥ siddha-vastir iti smṛtaḥ ।
dvi-pañca-mūla-tri-phalā-phala-bilvāni pācayet ।।

go-mūtre tena piṣṭaiś ca pāṭhā-vatsaka-toyadaiḥ ।
sa-phalaiḥ kṣaudra-tailābhyāṃ kṣāreṇa lavaṇena ca ।।

ṣāreṇa lavaṇena vā
yukto vastiḥ kapha-vyādhi-pāṇḍu-roga-viṣūciṣu ।
śukrānila-vibandheṣu vasty-āṭope ca pūjitaḥ ।।

asty-āṭopeṣu pūjitaḥ
mustā-pāṭhāmṛtairaṇḍa-balā-rāsnā-punarnavāḥ ।
mañjiṣṭhāragvadhośīra-trāyamāṇākṣa-rohiṇīḥ ।।

-balā-rāsnā-punarnavam -trāyamāṇākṣa-rohiṇi
kanīyaḥ pañca-mūlaṃ ca pālikaṃ madanāṣṭakam ।
jalāḍhake pacet tac ca pāda-śeṣaṃ parisrutam ।।

kṣīra-dvi-prastha-saṃyuktaṃ kṣīra-śeṣaṃ punaḥ pacet ।
sa-pāda-jāṅgala-rasaḥ sa-sarpir-madhu-saindhavaḥ ।।

piṣṭair yaṣṭī-miśi-śyāmā-kaliṅgaka-rasāñjanaiḥ ।
vastiḥ sukhoṣṇo māṃsāgni-bala-śukra-vivardhanaḥ ।।

vātāsṛṅ-moha-mehārśo-gulma-viṇ-mūtra-saṃgrahān ।
viṣama-jvara-vīsarpa-vardhmādhmāna-pravāhikāḥ ।।

āta-rakta-pramehārśo- ātāsṛṅ-meha-medo-'rśo- 
-gulma-viṇ-mūtra-saṃgraham
vaṅkṣaṇoru-kaṭī-kukṣi-manyā-śrotra-śiro-rujaḥ ।
hanyād asṛg-daronmāda-śopha-kāsāśma-kuṇḍalān ।।

cakṣuṣyaḥ putra-do rājā yāpanānāṃ rasāyanam ।
mṛgāṇāṃ laghu-vadrāṇāṃ daśa-mūlasya cāmbhasā ।।

āpanānāṃ rasāyanaḥ ṛgāṇāṃ laghu-babhrūṇāṃ ṛgāṇāṃ laghu-barhāṇāṃ ṛgāṇāṃ laghu-vaḍrāṇāṃ ṛgāṇāṃ laghu-vabhrāṇāṃ ṛgāṇāṃ laghu-babhrāṇāṃ 
ṛgāṇāṃ laghu-vargāṇāṃ
hapuṣā-miśi-gāṅgeyī-kalkair vāta-haraḥ param ।
nirūho aty-artha-vṛṣyaś ca mahā-sneha-samanvitaḥ ।।

-kalkair vāta-haraiḥ param -kalko vāta-haraḥ param
mayūraṃ pakṣa-pittāntra-pāda-viṭ-tuṇḍa-varjitam ।
laghunā pañca-mūlena pālikena samanvitam ।।

paktvā kṣīra-jale kṣīra-śeṣaṃ sa-ghṛta-mākṣikam ।
tad vidārī-kaṇā-yaṣṭī-śatāhvā-phala-kalka-vat ।।

-śatāhvā-phala-kalka-vān
vastir īṣat-paṭu-yutaḥ paramaṃ bala-śukra-kṛt ।
kalpaneyaṃ pṛthak kāryā tittiri-prabhṛtiṣv api ।।

aramaṃ bala-varṇa-kṛt
viṣkireṣu samasteṣu pratuda-prasaheṣu ca ।
jala-cāriṣu tad-vac ca matsyeṣu kṣīra-varjitā ।।

godhā-nakula-mārjāra-śalyakondura-jaṃ palam ।
pṛthag daśa-palaṃ kṣīre pañca-mūlaṃ ca sādhayet ।।

tat payaḥ phala-vaidehī-kalka-dvi-lavaṇānvitam ।
sa-sitā-taila-madhv-ājyo vastir yojyo rasāyanam ।।

a-sitā-taila-madhv-ājyaṃ a-sitā-taila-madhv-ājyaṃ
vyāyāma-mathitoraska-kṣīṇendriya-balaujasām ।
vibaddha-śukra-viṇ-mūtra-khuḍa-vāta-vikāriṇām ।।

ibandha-śukra-viṇ-mūtra-
gaja-vāji-ratha-kṣobha-bhagna-jarjaritātmanām ।
punar-nava-tvaṃ kurute vājī-karaṇam uttamam ।।

ājī-karaṇa-sat-tamam
siddhena payasā bhojyam ātmaguptoccaṭekṣuraiḥ ।
snehāṃś cā-yantraṇān siddhān siddha-dravyaiḥ prakalpayet ।।

nehāṃś cāḍhya-guṇān siddhān
doṣa-ghnāḥ sa-parīhārā vakṣyante sneha-vastayaḥ ।
daśa-mūlaṃ balāṃ rāsnām aśvagandhāṃ punarnavām ।।

oṣa-ghnā niṣ-parīhārā
guḍūcyairaṇḍa-bhūtīka-bhārgī-vṛṣaka-rohiṣam ।
śatāvarīṃ sahacaraṃ kākanāsāṃ palāṃśakam ।।

uḍūcyairaṇḍa-pūtīka- ākanāsāṃ palāṃśikam 
kākanāsāṃ palāṃśikām
yava-māṣātasī-kola-kulatthān prasṛtonmitān ।
vahe vipācya toyasya droṇa-śeṣeṇa tena ca ।।

pacet tailāḍhakaṃ peṣyair jīvanīyaiḥ palonmitaiḥ ।
anuvāsanam ity etat sarva-vāta-vikāra-nut ।।

acet tailāḍḥakaṃ kalkair arva-vāta-vikāra-jit
ānūpānāṃ vasā tad-vaj jīvanīyopasādhitā ।
śatāhvā-ciribilvāmlais tailaṃ siddhaṃ samīraṇe ।।

śatāhvā-yava-bilvāmlais ailaṃ tad-vat samīraṇe
saindhavenāgni-varṇena taptaṃ cānila-jid ghṛtam ।
jīvantīṃ madanaṃ medāṃ śrāvaṇīṃ madhukaṃ balām ।।

śatāhvarṣabhakau kṛṣṇāṃ kākanāsāṃ śatāvarīm ।
svaguptāṃ kṣīra-kākolīṃ karkaṭākhyāṃ śaṭhīṃ vacām ।।

piṣṭvā taila-ghṛtaṃ kṣīre sādhayet tac-catur-guṇe ।
bṛṃhaṇaṃ vāta-pitta-ghnaṃ bala-śukrāgni-vardhanam ।।

iṣṭvā tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣīre ādhayet ca catur-guṇe
rajaḥ-śukrāmaya-haraṃ putrīyaṃ cānuvāsanam ।
saindhavaṃ madanaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śatāhvā niculo vacā ।।

ajaḥ-śukrānila-haraṃ utrīyam anuvāsanam
hrīveraṃ madhukaṃ bhārgī devadāru sa-kaṭphalam ।
nāgaraṃ puṣkaraṃ medā cavikā citrakaḥ śaṭhī ।।

rīveraṃ padmakaṃ bhārgī
viḍaṅgātiviṣe śyāmā hareṇur nīlinī sthirā ।
bilvājamoda-capalā dantī rāsnā ca taiḥ samaiḥ ।।

iḍaṅgātiviṣā-śyāmā ilvājamodā-capalā ilvājamode 
capalā
sādhyam eraṇḍa-tailaṃ vā tailaṃ vā kapha-roga-nut ।
vardhmodāvarta-gulmārśaḥ-plīha-mehāḍhya-mārutān ।।

ādhyam eraṇḍa-jaṃ tailaṃ apha-vāta-ja-roga-nut
ānāham aśmarīṃ cāśu hanyāt tad anuvāsanam ।
sādhitaṃ pañca-mūlena tailaṃ bilvādinātha-vā ।।

kapha-ghnaṃ kalpayet tailaṃ dravyair vā kapha-ghātibhiḥ ।
phalair aṣṭa-guṇaiś cāmlaiḥ siddham anvāsanaṃ kaphe ।।

halair aṣṭa-guṇe cāmle
mṛdu-vasti-jaḍī-bhūte tīkṣṇo anyo vastir iṣyate ।
tīkṣṇair vikarṣite snigdho madhuraḥ śiśiro mṛduḥ ।।

ṛdu-vastau jaḍī-bhūte
tīkṣṇa-tvaṃ mūtra-pīlv-agni-lavaṇa-kṣāra-sarṣapaiḥ ।
prāpta-kālaṃ vidhātavyaṃ kṣīrājyādyais tu mārdavam ।।

īkṣṇa-tvaṃ mūtra-bilvāgni- ṣīrājyādyaiś ca mārdavam ṣīrādyaiś caiva mārdavam 
hṛta-kṣīrais tu mārdavam
bala-kāla-roga-doṣa-prakṛtīḥ pravibhajya yojito vastiḥ ।
svaiḥ svair auṣadha-vargaiḥ svān svān rogān nivartayati ।।

-prakṛtīḥ pravivīkṣya yojito vastiḥ vān svān doṣān nivartayati
uṣṇārtānāṃ śītāñ chītārtānāṃ tathā sukhoṣṇāṃś ca ।
tad-yogyauṣadha-yuktān vastīn saṃtarkya yuñjīta ।।

vastīn na bṛṃhaṇīyān dadyād vyādhiṣu viśodhanīyeṣu ।
medasvino viśodhyā ye ca narāḥ kuṣṭha-mehārtāḥ ।।

adyād vyādhiṣu ca śodhanīyeṣu
na kṣīṇa-kṣata-dur-bala-mūrchita-kṛśa-śuṣka-śuddha-dehānām ।
dadyād viśodhanīyān doṣa-nibaddhāyuṣo ye ca ।।

kalpasthāna
a-snigdha-svinna-dehasya guru-koṣṭhasya yojitaḥ ।
śīto alpa-sneha-lavaṇa-dravya-mātro ghano api vā ।।

-drava-mātro ghano api vā
vastiḥ saṃkṣobhya taṃ doṣaṃ dur-bala-tvād a-nirharan ।
karoty a-yogaṃ tena syād vāta-mūtra-śakṛd-grahaḥ ।।

astiḥ saṃstabhya taṃ doṣaṃ
nābhi-vasti-rujā dāho hṛl-lepaḥ śvayathur gude ।
kaṇḍūr gaṇḍāni vaivarṇyam a-ratir vahni-mārdavam ।।

ābhi-vasti-rujānāho aṇḍūr gaṇḍāti-vaivarṇyam aṇḍūr 
gaṇḍākṣi-vaivarṇyam
kvātha-dvayaṃ prāg-vihitaṃ madhya-doṣe atisāriṇi ।
uṣṇasya tasmād ekasya tatra pānaṃ praśasyate ।।

atra pānaṃ vidhīyate
phala-vartyas tathā svedāḥ kālaṃ jñātvā virecanam ।
bilva-mūla-trivṛd-dāru-yava-kola-kulattha-vān ।।

surādi-mūtra-vān vastiḥ sa-prāk-peṣyas tam ānayet ।
yukto alpa-vīryo doṣāḍhye rūkṣe krūrāśaye atha-vā ।।

urādi-māṃs tatra vastiḥ
vastir doṣāvṛto ruddha-mārgo rundhyāt samīraṇam ।
sa vi-mārgo anilaḥ kuryād ādhmānaṃ marma-pīḍanam ।।

vidāhaṃ guda-koṣṭhasya muṣka-vaṅkṣaṇa-vedanām ।
ruṇaddhi hṛdayaṃ śūlair itaś cetaś ca dhāvati ।।

sv-abhyakta-svinna-gātrasya tatra vartiṃ prayojayet ।
bilvādiś ca nirūhaḥ syāt pīlu-sarṣapa-mūtra-vān ।।

bhyakta-svinna-gātrasya v-abhyakta-svinna-gātrāya 
sv-abhyakta-svinna-dehasya
saralāmaradārubhyāṃ sādhitaṃ cānuvāsanam ।
kurvato vega-saṃrodhaṃ pīḍito vāti-mātrayā ।।

ādhitaṃ vānuvāsanam īḍitaś cāti-mātrayā
a-snigdha-lavaṇoṣṇo vā vastir alpo alpa-bheṣajaḥ ।
mṛdur vā mārutenordhvaṃ vikṣipto mukha-nāsikāt ।।

nireti mūrchā-hṛl-lāsa-tṛḍ-dāhādīn pravartayan ।
mūrchā-vikāraṃ dṛṣṭvāsya siñcec chītāmbunā mukham ।।

-tṛḍ-dāhādīn prakalpayet -tṛḍ-dāhādīn pravartayet
vyajed ā-klama-nāśāc ca prāṇāyāmaṃ ca kārayet ।
pṛṣṭha-pārśvodaraṃ mṛjyāt karair uṣṇair adho-mukham ।।

ījet klama-vināśāc ca ījed ā-klama-nāśāc ca ījyed ā-klama-nāśāc ca 
ṛṣṭha-pārśvodaraṃ mṛdyāt
keśeṣūtkṣipya dhunvīta bhīṣayed vyāla-daṃṣṭribhiḥ ।
śastrolkā-rāja-puruṣair vastir eti tathā hy adhaḥ ।।

hāyayed vyāla-daṃṣṭribhiḥv hāpayed vyāla-daṃṣṭribhiḥ
pāṇi-vastrair galāpīḍaṃ kuryān na mriyate tathā ।
prāṇodāna-nirodhād dhi su-prasiddha-tarāyanaḥ ।।

apānaḥ pavano vastiṃ tam āśv evāpakarṣati ।
kuṣṭha-kramuka-kalkaṃ ca pāyayetāmla-saṃyutam ।।

athāśv evāpakarṣati uṣṭha-kramuka-kalkaṃ vā 
pāyayed amla-saṃyutam
auṣṇyāt taikṣṇyāt sara-tvāc ca vastiṃ so asyānulomayet ।
go-mūtreṇa trivṛt-pathyā-kalkaṃ vādho-'nulomanam ।।

-kalkaṃ cādho-'nulomanam
pakvāśaya-sthite svinne nirūho dāśamūlikaḥ ।
yava-kola-kulatthaiś ca vidheyo mūtra-sādhitaiḥ ।।

idheyo mūtra-sādhitaḥ
vastir go-mūtra-siddhair vā sāmṛtā-vaṃśa-pallavaiḥ ।
pūti-karañja-tvak-pattra-śaṭhī-devāhva-rohiṣaiḥ ।।

sa-taila-guḍa-sindhūttho virekauṣadha-kalka-vān ।
bilvādi-pañca-mūlena siddho vastir uraḥ-sthite ।।

śiraḥ-sthe nāvanaṃ dhūmaḥ pracchādyaṃ sarṣapaiḥ śiraḥ ।
vastir aty-uṣṇa-tīkṣṇāmla-ghano ati-sveditasya vā ।।

alpe doṣe mṛdau koṣṭhe prayukto vā punaḥ punaḥ ।
ati-yoga-tvam āpanno bhavet kukṣi-rujā-karaḥ ।।

virecanāti-yogena sa tulyākṛti-sādhanaḥ ।
vastiḥ kṣārāmla-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-lavaṇaḥ paittikasya vā ।।

-lavaṇaḥ paittikasya ca
gudaṃ dahan likhan kṣiṇvan karoty asya parisravam ।
sa vidagdhaṃ sravaty asraṃ varṇaiḥ pittaṃ ca bhūribhiḥ ।।

aroty asra-parisravam
bahu-śaś cāti-vegena mohaṃ gacchati so a-sakṛt ।
rakta-pittātisāra-ghnī kriyā tatra praśasyate ।।

ahu-śaś cāti-yogena ohaṃ gacchati cā-sakṛt ohaṃ 
gacchati vā-sakṛt
dāhādiṣu trivṛt-kalkaṃ mṛdvīkā-vāriṇā pibet ।
tad dhi pitta-śakṛd-vātān hṛtvā dāhādikāñ jayet ।।

atvā dāhādikāñ jayet
viśuddhaś ca pibec chītāṃ yavāgūṃ śarkarā-yutām ।
yuñjyād vāti-viriktasya kṣīṇa-viṭkasya bhojanam ।।

avāgūṃ śarkarānvitām
māṣa-yūṣeṇa kulmāṣān pānaṃ dadhy atha-vā surām ।
siddhir vasty-āpadām evaṃ sneha-vastes tu vakṣyate ।।

neha-vastiṣu vakṣyate neha-kalpas tu vakṣyate
śīto alpo vādhike vāte pitte aty-uṣṇaḥ kaphe mṛduḥ ।
ati-bhukte gurur varcaḥ-saṃcaye alpa-balas tathā ।।

dattas tair āvṛtaḥ sneho nāyāty abhibhavād api ।
stambhoru-sadanādhmāna-jvara-śūlāṅga-mardanaiḥ ।।

āyāty abhibhavād adhaḥ
pārśva-rug-veṣṭanair vidyād vāyunā sneham āvṛtam ।
snigdhāmla-lavaṇoṣṇais taṃ rāsnā-pītadru-tailikaiḥ ।।

sauvīraka-surā-kola-kulattha-yava-sādhitaiḥ ।
nirūhair nirharet samyak sa-mūtraiḥ pāñcamūlikaiḥ ।।

auvīraka-surāṅkolla- a-mūtraiḥ pāñcamaulikaiḥ
tābhyām eva ca tailābhyāṃ sāyaṃ bhukte anuvāsayet ।
tṛḍ-dāha-rāga-saṃmoha-vaivarṇya-tamaka-jvaraiḥ ।।

ābhyām eva tu tailābhyāṃ ailābhyām eva tābhyāṃ vā
vidyāt pittāvṛtaṃ svādu-tiktais taṃ vastibhir haret ।
tandrā-śīta-jvarālasya-prasekā-ruci-gauravaiḥ ।।

-tiktais taṃ ca vinirharet
saṃmūrchā-glānibhir vidyāc chleṣmaṇā sneham āvṛtam ।
kaṣāya-tikta-kaṭukaiḥ surā-mūtropasādhitaiḥ ।।

a-mūrchā-glānibhir vidyāc urā-mūtraiḥ prasādhitaiḥ 
surā-go-mūtra-sādhitaiḥ
phala-taila-yutaiḥ sāmlair vastibhis taṃ vinirharet ।
chardi-mūrchā-ruci-glāni-śūla-nidrāṅga-mardanaiḥ ।।

-śūla-tandrāṅga-mardanaiḥ
āma-liṅgaiḥ sa-dāhais taṃ vidyād aty-aśanāvṛtam ।
kaṭūnāṃ lavaṇānāṃ ca kvāthaiś cūrṇaiś ca pācanam ।।

idyād āmāvṛtaṃ tu tam
mṛdur virekaḥ sarvaṃ ca tatrāma-vihitaṃ hitam ।
viṇ-mūtrānila-saṅgārti-guru-tvādhmāna-hṛd-grahaiḥ ।।

snehaṃ viḍ-āvṛtaṃ jñātvā sneha-svedaiḥ sa-vartibhiḥ ।
śyāmā-bilvādi-siddhaiś ca nirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ ।।

nirhared vidhinā samyag udāvarta-hareṇa ca ।
a-bhukte śūna-pāyau vā peyā-mātrāśitasya vā ।।

dāvarta-hareṇa vā eyā-mātrāśitasya ca
gude praṇihitaḥ sneho vegād dhāvaty an-āvṛtaḥ ।
ūrdhvaṃ kāyaṃ tataḥ kaṇṭhād ūrdhvebhyaḥ khebhya ety api ।।

ūrdhva-kāyaṃ tataḥ kaṇṭhād
mūtra-śyāmā-trivṛt-siddho yava-kola-kulattha-vān ।
tat-siddha-tailo deyaḥ syān nirūhaḥ sānuvāsanaḥ ।।

kaṇṭhād āgacchataḥ stambha-kaṇṭha-graha-virecanaiḥ ।
chardi-ghnībhiḥ kriyābhiś ca tasya kuryān nibarhaṇam ।।

nā-pakvaṃ praṇayet snehaṃ gudaṃ sa hy upalimpati ।
tataḥ kuryāt sa-ruṅ-moha-kaṇḍū-śophān kriyātra ca ।।

ā-pakvaṃ snehayet snehaṃ ataḥ kuryāt sa-tṛṇ-moha- 
sa kuryāt sakthi-ruṅ-moha-
tīkṣṇo vastis tathā tailam arka-pattra-rase śṛtam ।
an-ucchvāsya tu baddhe vā datte niḥśeṣa eva vā ।।

n-ucchvāsya nu baddhe vā n-ucchvāsyānubaddhe vā 
datte niḥśeṣa eva ca
praviśya kṣubhito vāyuḥ śūla-toda-karo bhavet ।
tatrābhyaṅgo gude svedo vāta-ghnāny aśanāni ca ।।

āta-ghnāny aśanāny atha
drutaṃ praṇīte niṣkṛṣṭe sahasotkṣipta eva vā ।
syāt kaṭī-guda-jaṅghoru-vasti-stambhārti-bhedanam ।।

bhojanaṃ tatra vāta-ghnaṃ svedābhyaṅgāḥ sa-vastayaḥ ।
pīḍyamāne antarā mukte gude pratihato anilaḥ ।।

uraḥ-śiro-rujaṃ sādam ūrvoś ca janayed balī ।
vastiḥ syāt tatra bilvādi-phala-śyāmādi-mūtra-vān ।।

astiḥ syāt tatra bilvādiḥ hala-śyāmādi-mūtra-vān
ati-prapīḍitaḥ koṣṭhe tiṣṭhaty āyāti vā galam ।
tatra vastir virekaś ca gala-pīḍādi karma ca ।।

iṣṭhann āyāti vā galam
vamanādyair viśuddhaṃ ca kṣāma-deha-balānalam ।
yathāṇḍaṃ taruṇaṃ pūrṇaṃ taila-pātraṃ yathā tathā ।।

armabhir vamanādyaiś ca amanādyair viśuddhaṃ tu
bhiṣak prayatnato rakṣet sarvasmād apacārataḥ ।
dadyān madhura-hṛdyāni tato amla-lavaṇau rasau ।।

arvasmād apavādataḥ
svādu-tiktau tato bhūyaḥ kaṣāya-kaṭukau tataḥ ।
anyo-'nya-praty-anīkānāṃ rasānāṃ snigdha-rūkṣayoḥ ।।

vyatyāsād upayogena kramāt taṃ prakṛtiṃ nayet ।
sarvaṃ-sahaḥ sthira-balo vijñeyaḥ prakṛtiṃ gataḥ ।।

kalpasthāna
dhanve sādhāraṇe deśe same san-mṛttike śucau ।
śmaśāna-caityāyatana-śvabhra-valmīka-varjite ।।

hanva-sādhāraṇe deśe śmaśāna-caityādyatana-
mṛdau pradakṣiṇa-jale kuśa-rohiṣa-saṃstṛte ।
a-phāla-kṛṣṭe an-ākrānte pādapair bala-vat-taraiḥ ।।

uśa-rohiṣa-saṃskṛte
śasyate bheṣajaṃ jātaṃ yuktaṃ varṇa-rasādibhiḥ ।
jantv-a-jagdhaṃ davā-dagdham a-vidagdhaṃ ca vaikṛtaiḥ ।।

antv-a-juṣṭaṃ davā-dagdham -vijagdhaṃ ca vaikṛtaiḥ
bhūtaiś chāyātapāmbv-ādyair yathā-kālaṃ ca sevitam ।
avagāḍha-mahā-mūlam udīcīṃ diśam āśritam ।।

dīcīṃ diśam āsthitam
mahendra-rāma-kṛṣṇānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ gavām api ।
tapasā tejasā vāpi praśāmyadhvaṃ śivāya vai ।।

tapasāṃ tejasāṃ vāpi praśāmyadhvaṃ śamāya vai mantreṇānena mati-mān sarvam apy auṣadhaṃ nayet ।।

atha kalyāṇa-caritaḥ śrāddhaḥ śucir upoṣitaḥ ।
gṛhṇīyād auṣadhaṃ su-sthaṃ sthitaṃ kāle ca kalpayet ।।

sa-kṣīraṃ tad a-saṃpattāv an-atikrānta-vatsaram ।
ṛte guḍa-ghṛta-kṣaudra-dhānya-kṛṣṇā-viḍaṅgataḥ ।।

ṛte ghṛta-guḍa-kṣaudra-
payo bāṣkayaṇaṃ grāhyaṃ viṇ-mūtraṃ tac ca nī-rujām ।
vayo-bala-vatāṃ dhātu-piccha-śṛṅga-khurādikam ।।

iṇ-mūtraṃ tac ca nī-ruji iṇ-mūtraṃ tac ca nī-rujam -puccha-śṛṅga-khurādikam 
-pitta-śṛṅga-khurādikam
kaṣāya-yonayaḥ pañca rasā lavaṇa-varjitāḥ ।
rasaḥ kalkaḥ śṛtaḥ śītaḥ phāṇṭaś ceti prakalpanā ।।

hāṇṭaś ceti prakalpanāḥ
pañca-dhaiva kaṣāyāṇāṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ balādhikā ।
sadyaḥ-samuddhṛtāt kṣuṇṇād yaḥ sravet paṭa-pīḍitāt ।।

añca caiva kaṣāyāṇāṃ ūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ balādhikāḥ ūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ balāvahāḥ 
adyaḥ-samuddhṛta-kṣuṇṇād aḥ sravet paṭa-pīḍanāt
sva-rasaḥ sa samuddiṣṭaḥ kalkaḥ piṣṭo dravāplutaḥ ।
cūrṇo a-plutaḥ śṛtaḥ kvāthaḥ śīto rātriṃ drave sthitaḥ ।।

śīto rātrau drave sthitaḥ
sadyo-'bhiṣuta-pūtas tu phāṇṭas tan-māna-kalpane ।
yuñjyād vyādhy-ādi-balatas tathā ca vacanaṃ muneḥ ।।

adyo-'bhikṣuṇṇa-pūtas tu
mātrāyā na vyavasthāsti vyādhiṃ koṣṭhaṃ balaṃ vayaḥ ।
ālocya deśa-kālau ca yojyā tad-vac ca kalpanā ।।

ātrāyā nāsty avasthānaṃ oṣam agniṃ balaṃ vayaḥ
madhyaṃ tu mānaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ sva-rasasya catuḥ-palam ।
peṣyasya karṣam āloḍyaṃ tad dravasya pala-traye ।।

adhya-mānaṃ vinirdiṣṭaṃ
kvāthaṃ dravya-pale kuryāt prasthārdhaṃ pāda-śeṣitam ।
śītaṃ pale palaiḥ ṣaḍbhiś caturbhis tu tato aparam ।।

aturbhiś ca tato aparam aturbhis tu tataḥ param
sneha-pāke tv a-mānoktau catur-guṇa-vivardhitam ।
kalka-sneha-dravaṃ yojyam adhīte śaunakaḥ punaḥ ।।

snehe sidhyati śuddhāmbu-niḥkvātha-sva-rasaiḥ kramāt ।
kalkasya yojayed aṃśaṃ caturthaṃ ṣaṣṭham aṣṭamam ।।

pṛthak sneha-samaṃ dadyāt pañca-prabhṛti tu dravam ।
nāṅgulī-grāhi-tā kalke na snehe agnau sa-śabda-tā ।।

ravaṃ tu pañca-prabhṛti ṛthak sneha-samaṃ kṣipet
śuṣka-dravyaṃ yadā na syāt tadā sadyaḥ-samuddhṛtam ।
dvi-guṇaṃ tat prayoktavyaṃ kuḍavādi dravaṃ tathā ।।

varṇādi-saṃpac ca yadā tadainaṃ śīghram āharet ।
ghṛtasya phenopaśamas tailasya tu tad-udbhavaḥ ।।

c tailasya ca tad-udbhavaḥ
lehasya tantu-mat-tāpsu majjanaṃ saraṇaṃ na ca ।
pākas tu tri-vidho mandaś cikkaṇaḥ khara-cikkaṇaḥ ।।

ajjanaṃ śaraṇaṃ na ca
mandaḥ kalka-same kiṭṭe cikkaṇo madanopame ।
kiñ-cit sīdati kṛṣṇe ca vartya-māne ca paścimaḥ ।।

arti-māne ca paścimaḥ artamāne ca paścimaḥ 
vartamāne tu paścimaḥ
dagdho ata ūrdhvaṃ niṣkāryaḥ syād āmas tv agni-sāda-kṛt ।
mṛdur nasye kharo abhyaṅge pāne vastau ca cikkaṇaḥ ।।

śāṇaṃ pāṇi-talaṃ muṣṭiṃ kuḍavaṃ prastham āḍhakam ।
droṇaṃ vahaṃ ca krama-śo vijānīyāc catur-guṇam ।।

dvi-guṇaṃ yojayed ārdraṃ kuḍavādi tathā dravam ।
peṣaṇāloḍane vāri sneha-pāke ca nir-drave ।।

kalpayet sadṛśān bhāgān pramāṇaṃ yatra noditam ।
kalkī-kuryāc ca bhaiṣajyam a-nirūpita-kalpanam ।।

aṅgān-uktau tu mūlaṃ syād a-prasiddhau tad eva tu ।
dvau śāṇau vaṭakaḥ kolaṃ badaraṃ draṅkṣaṇaś ca tau ।।

-nirdiṣṭā-prasiddheṣu ūlaṃ grāhyaṃ tvag-ādiṣu 
dvau śāṇau vaṭakaḥ kolo
ṣaḍ vaṃśyas tu marīciḥ syāt ṣaṇ marīcyas tu sarṣapaḥ ।
taṇḍulaḥ sarṣapās tv aṣṭau dhānya-māṣas tu tau yavaḥ ।।

dhānya-māṣaś ca tau yavaḥ tāv aṇḍikā caturbhis tair māṣakaḥ śāṇakas tathā ।।

tāvanto gaditā māṣāḥ tais turyair guñjakā māṣas 
śāṇo ayaṃ munibhiḥ smṛtaḥ turyābhiḥ śāṇakaḥ smṛtaḥ
akṣaṃ picuḥ pāṇi-talaṃ suvarṇaṃ kavaḍa-grahaḥ ।
karṣo biḍāla-padakaṃ tindukaḥ pāṇi-mānikā ।।

uvarṇaṃ kavaḍa-graham indukaṃ pāṇi-mānikā
śabdānya-tvam a-bhinne arthe śuktir aṣṭamikā picū ।
palaṃ prakuñco bilvaṃ ca muṣṭir āmraṃ caturthikā ।।

śabdān evam a-bhinne arthe śabdā hy amī a-bhinne arthe
dve pale prasṛtas tau dvāv añjalis tau tu mānikā ।
āḍhakaṃ bhājanaṃ kaṃso droṇaḥ kumbho ghaṭo armaṇam ।।

ve pale prasṛtis tau dvāv
tulā pala-śataṃ tāni viṃśatir bhāra ucyate ।
himavad-vindhya-śailābhyāṃ prāyo vyāptā vasundharā ।।

ulā pala-śataṃ tāsāṃ saumyaṃ pathyaṃ ca tatrādyam āgneyaṃ vaindhyam auṣadham ।।

ū̆saumyaṃ tatrādyam āgneyaṃ ū̆vaindhyam auṣadham īritam

uttarasthāna
jāta-mātraṃ viśodhyolbād bālaṃ saindhava-sarpiṣā ।
prasūti-kleśitaṃ cānu balā-tailena secayet ।।

aśmanor vādanaṃ cāsya karṇa-mūle samācaret ।
athāsya dakṣiṇe karṇe mantram uccārayed imam ।।

aṅgād aṅgāt saṃbhavasi hṛdayād abhijāyase ।
ātmā vai putra-nāmāsi saṃjīva śaradāṃ śatam ।।

aṃjīva śaradaḥ śatam
śatāyuḥ śata-varṣo asi dīrgham āyur avāpnuhi ।
nakṣatrāṇi diśo rātrir ahaś ca tvābhirakṣatu ।।

haś catvāri rakṣatu
svasthī-bhūtasya nābhiṃ ca sūtreṇa catur-aṅgulāt ।
baddhvordhvaṃ vardhayitvā ca grīvāyām avasañjayet ।।

addhvordhvaṃ vardhayitvā tu rīvāyām avasajjayet
nābhiṃ ca kuṣṭha-tailena secayet snāpayed anu ।
kṣīri-vṛkṣa-kaṣāyeṇa sarva-gandhodakena vā ।।

ābhiṃ tu kuṣṭha-tailena ecayet snapayed anu
koṣṇena tapta-rajata-tapanīya-nimajjanaiḥ ।
tato dakṣiṇa-tarjanyā tālūnnamyāvaguṇṭhayet ।।

śirasi sneha-picunā prāśyaṃ cāsya prayojayet ।
hareṇu-mātraṃ medhāyur-balārtham abhimantritam ।।

rāśaṃ cāsya prayojayet
aindrī-brāhmī-vacā-śaṅkhapuṣpī-kalkaṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu ।
cāmīkara-vacā-brāhmī-tāpya-pathyā rajī-kṛtāḥ ।।

-kuṣṭha-pathyā rajī-kṛtāḥ
lihyān madhu-ghṛtopetā hema-dhātrī-rajo atha-vā ।
garbhāmbhaḥ saindhava-vatā sarpiṣā vāmayet tataḥ ।।

arbhāmbhaḥ saindhava-vacā- -sarpiṣā vāmayet tataḥ
prājāpatyena vidhinā jāta-karmāṇi kārayet ।
sirāṇāṃ hṛdaya-sthānāṃ vivṛta-tvāt prasūtitaḥ ।।

tṛtīye ahni caturthe vā strīṇāṃ stanyaṃ pravartate ।
prathame divase tasmāt tri-kālaṃ madhu-sarpiṣī ।।

anantā-miśrite mantra-pāvite prāśayec chiśum ।
dvitīye lakṣmaṇā-siddhaṃ tṛtīye ca ghṛtaṃ tataḥ ।।

prāṅ-niṣiddha-stanasyāsya tat-pāṇi-tala-saṃmitam ।
stanyānu-pānaṃ dvau kālau nava-nītaṃ prayojayet ।।

mātur eva pibet stanyaṃ tad dhy alaṃ deha-vṛddhaye ।
stanya-dhātryāv ubhe kārye tad-a-saṃpadi vatsale ।।

at paraṃ deha-vṛddhaye
a-vyaṅge brahma-cāriṇyau varṇa-prakṛtitaḥ same ।
nī-ruje madhya-vayasau jīvad-vatse na lolupe ।।

hitāhāra-vihāreṇa yatnād upacarec ca te ।
śuk-krodha-laṅghanāyāsāḥ stanya-nāśasya hetavaḥ ।।

stanyasya sīdhu-varjyāni madyāny ānūpa-jā rasāḥ ।
kṣīraṃ kṣīriṇya oṣadhyaḥ śokādeś ca viparyayaḥ ।।

ṣīraṃ kṣīriṇy auṣadhayaḥ
viruddhāhāra-bhuktāyāḥ kṣudhitāyā vi-cetasaḥ ।
praduṣṭa-dhātor garbhiṇyāḥ stanyaṃ roga-karaṃ śiśoḥ ।।

iruddhāhāra-ceṣṭāyāḥ
stanyā-bhāve payaś chāgaṃ gavyaṃ vā tad-guṇaṃ pibet ।
hrasvena pañca-mūlena sthirābhyāṃ vā sitā-yutam ।।

ūlaiḥ siddhaṃ bṛhaty-ādyaiḥ
ṣaṣṭhīṃ niśāṃ viśeṣeṇa kṛta-rakṣā-bali-kriyāḥ ।
jāgṛyur bāndhavās tasya dadhataḥ paramāṃ mudam ।।

daśame divase pūrṇe vidhibhiḥ sva-kulocitaiḥ ।
kārayet sūtikotthānaṃ nāma bālasya cārcitam ।।

idhi-vat sva-kulocitaiḥ
bibhrato aṅgair manohvāla-rocanāguru-candanam ।
nakṣatra-devatā-yuktaṃ bāndhavaṃ vā samākṣaram ।।

tataḥ prakṛti-bhedokta-rūpair āyuḥ-parīkṣaṇam ।
prāg-udak-śirasaḥ kuryād bālasya jñāna-vān bhiṣak ।।

śuci-dhautopadhānāni nir-valīni mṛdūni ca ।
śayyāstaraṇa-vāsāṃsi rakṣo-ghnair dhūpitāni ca ।।

kāko viśastaḥ śastaś ca dhūpane trivṛtānvitaḥ ।
jīvat-khaḍgādi-śṛṅgotthān sadā bālaḥ śubhān maṇīn ।।

aṅko viśastaḥ śastaś ca īvat-khaḍgādi-śṛṅga-sthān
dhārayed auṣadhīḥ śreṣṭhāḥ brāhmy-aindrī-jīvakādikāḥ ।
hastābhyāṃ grīvayā mūrdhnā viśeṣāt satataṃ vacām ।।

hārayec cauṣadhīḥ śreṣṭhā hārayed auṣadhīś ceṣṭā
āyur-medhā-smṛti-svāsthya-karīṃ rakṣo-'bhirakṣiṇīm ।
ṣaṭ-saptāṣṭama-māseṣu nī-rujasya śubhe ahani ।।

ṣaṭ-saptāṣṭasu māseṣu
karṇau himāgame vidhyed dhātry-aṅka-sthasya sāntvayan ।
prāg dakṣiṇaṃ kumārasya bhiṣag vāmaṃ tu yoṣitaḥ ।।

dakṣiṇena dadhat sūcīṃ pālīm anyena pāṇinā ।
madhyataḥ karṇa-pīṭhasya kiñ-cid gaṇḍāśrayaṃ prati ।।

jarāyu-mātra-pracchanne ravi-raśmy-avabhāsite ।
ghṛtasya niś-calaṃ samyag alaktaka-rasāṅkite ।।

vidhyed daiva-kṛte cchidre sakṛd evarju lāghavāt ।
nordhvaṃ na pārśvato nādhaḥ sirās tatra hi saṃśritāḥ ।।

kālikā-marmarī-raktās tad-vyadhād rāga-rug-jvarāḥ ।
sa-śopha-dāha-saṃrambha-manyā-stambhāpatānakāḥ ।।

ad-bādhād rāga-rug-jvarāḥ
teṣāṃ yathāmayaṃ kuryād vibhajyāśu cikitsitam ।
sthāne vyadhān na rudhiraṃ na rug-rāgādi-saṃbhavaḥ ।।

thāna-vyadhān na rudhiraṃ
snehāktaṃ sūcy-anusyūtaṃ sūtraṃ cānu nidhāpayet ।
āma-tailena siñcec ca bahalāṃ tad-vad ārayā ।।

vidhyet pālīṃ hita-bhujaḥ saṃcāryātha sthavīyasī ।
vartis try-ahāt tato rūḍhaṃ vardhayeta śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।।

aṃcāryānyā sthavīyasī artis try-ahāt tato rūḍhāṃ
athainaṃ jāta-daśanaṃ krameṇāpanayet stanāt ।
pūrvoktaṃ yojayet kṣīram annaṃ ca laghu bṛṃhaṇam ।।

āta-dantaṃ śiśuṃ śīte rama-śo apanayet stanāt
priyāla-majja-madhuka-madhu-lāja-sitopalaiḥ ।
apa-stanasya saṃyojyaḥ prīṇano modakaḥ śiśoḥ ।।

dīpano bāla-bilvailā-śarkarā-lāja-saktubhiḥ ।
saṃgrāhī dhātakī-puṣpa-śarkarā-lāja-tarpaṇaiḥ ।।

rogāṃś cāsya jayet saumyair bheṣajair a-viṣādakaiḥ ।
anya-trātyayikād vyādher virekaṃ su-tarāṃ tyajet ।।

heṣajair a-viṣādikaiḥ heṣajair a-vipādikaiḥ heṣajair 
a-vipādakaiḥ
trāsayen nā-vidheyaṃ taṃ trastaṃ gṛhṇanti hi grahāḥ ।
vastra-vātāt para-sparśāt pālayel laṅghanāc ca tam ।।

rāsayen nā-vidheyaṃ ca astra-pātāt khara-sparśāt astra-pātāt para-sparśāt 
ālayel laṅghitāc ca tam
brāhmī-siddhārthaka-vacā-śārivā-kuṣṭha-saindhavaiḥ ।
sa-kaṇaiḥ sādhitaṃ pītaṃ vāṅ-medhā-smṛti-kṛd ghṛtam ।।

āyuṣyaṃ pāpma-rakṣo-ghnaṃ bhūtonmāda-nibarhaṇam ।
vacendulekhā-maṇḍūkī-śaṅkhapuṣpī-śatāvarīḥ ।।

acendulekhā maṇḍūkī śaṅkhapuṣpī śatāvarī
brahmasomāmṛtā-brāhmīḥ kalkī-kṛtya palāṃśikāḥ ।
aṣṭāṅgaṃ vipacet sarpiḥ prasthaṃ kṣīra-catur-guṇam ।।

rahmasomāṃrtā brāhmī alkī-kṛtya palāṃśikaiḥ 
prasthaṃ kṣīraṃ catur-guṇam
tat pītaṃ dhanyam āyuṣyaṃ vāṅ-medhā-smṛti-buddhi-kṛt ।
ajā-kṣīrābhayā-vyoṣa-pāṭhogrā-śigru-saindhavaiḥ ।।

āṅ-medhā-smṛti-kṛt param āṅ-medhā-smṛti-vahni-kṛt 
-pāṭhogrā-śakra-saindhavaiḥ
siddhaṃ sārasvataṃ sarpir vāṅ-medhā-smṛti-vahni-kṛt ।
vacāmṛtā-śaṭhī-pathyā-śaṅkhinī-vella-nāgaraiḥ ।।

āṅ-medhā-smṛti-buddhi-kṛt acāmṛtā-varī-pathyā-
apāmārgeṇa ca ghṛtaṃ sādhitaṃ pūrva-vad guṇaiḥ ।
hema śveta-vacā kuṣṭham arkapuṣpī sa-kāñcanā ।।

ema śveta-vacā kuṣṭhaṃ śaṅkhapuṣpī sa-kāñcanā 
śaṅkhapuṣpī sa-rocanā
hema matsyākṣakaḥ śaṅkhaḥ kaiḍaryaḥ kanakaṃ vacā ।
catvāra ete pādoktāḥ prāśā madhu-ghṛta-plutāḥ ।।

ema matsyākṣakaḥ phañjī aiḍaryaṃ kanakaṃ vacā 
prāśyā madhu-ghṛta-plutāḥ
varṣaṃ līḍhā vapur-medhā-bala-varṇa-karāḥ śubhāḥ ।
vacā-yaṣṭy-āhva-sindhūttha-pathyā-nāgara-dīpyakaiḥ ।।

śudhyate vāg ghavir-līḍhaiḥ sa-kuṣṭha-kaṇa-jīrakaiḥ ।।
ū̆śudhyate vāg ghṛtālīḍhaiḥ

uttarasthāna
tri-vidhaḥ kathito bālaḥ kṣīrānnobhaya-vartanaḥ ।
svāsthyaṃ tābhyām a-duṣṭābhyāṃ duṣṭābhyāṃ roga-saṃbhavaḥ ।।

yad adbhir eka-tāṃ yāti na ca doṣair adhiṣṭhitam ।
tad viśuddhaṃ payo vātād duṣṭaṃ tu plavate ambhasi ।।

uṣṭaṃ tu plavate jale
kaṣāyaṃ phenilaṃ rūkṣaṃ varco-mūtra-vibandha-kṛt ।
pittād uṣṇāmla-kaṭukaṃ pīta-rājy apsu dāha-kṛt ।।

kaphāt sa-lavaṇaṃ sāndraṃ jale majjati picchilam ।
saṃsṛṣṭa-liṅgaṃ saṃsargāt tri-liṅgaṃ sāṃnipātikam ।।

yathā-sva-liṅgāṃs tad vyādhīn janayaty upayojitam ।
śiśos tīkṣṇam abhīkṣṇaṃ ca rodanāl lakṣayed rujam ।।

śiśos tīkṣṇam a-tīkṣṇaṃ ca
sa yaṃ spṛśed bhṛśaṃ deśaṃ yatra ca sparśanā-kṣamaḥ ।
tatra vidyād rujaṃ mūrdhni rujaṃ cākṣi-nimīlanāt ।।

vayaṃ spṛśed bhṛśaṃ deśaṃ atra ca sparśanā-kṣamam
hṛdi jihvauṣṭha-daśana-śvāsa-muṣṭi-nipīḍanaiḥ ।
koṣṭhe vibandha-vamathu-stana-daṃśāntra-kūjanaiḥ ।।

-śvāsa-muṣṭi-nipīḍitaiḥ -stanya-dveṣāntra-kūjanaiḥ
ādhmāna-pṛṣṭha-namana-jaṭharonnamanair api ।
vastau guhye ca viṇ-mūtra-saṅgottrāsa-dig-īkṣaṇaiḥ ।।

atha dhātryāḥ kriyāṃ kuryād yathā-doṣaṃ yathāmayam ।
tatra vātātmake stanye daśa-mūlaṃ try-ahaṃ pibet ।।

atha-vāgni-vacā-pāṭhā-kaṭukā-kuṣṭha-dīpyakam ।
sa-bhārgī-dāru-sarala-vṛścikālī-kaṇoṣaṇam ।।

tataḥ pibed anya-tamaṃ vāta-vyādhi-haraṃ ghṛtam ।
anu cāccha-surām evaṃ snigdhāṃ mṛdu virecayet ।।

āta-vyādhi-hitaṃ ghṛtam
vasti-karma tataḥ kuryāt svedādīṃś cānilāpahān ।
rāsnājamodā-sarala-devadāru-rajo-'nvitam ।।

bālo lihyād ghṛtaṃ tair vā vipakvaṃ sa-sitopalam ।
pitta-duṣṭe amṛtābhīru-paṭolī-nimba-candanam ।।

dhātrī kumāraś ca pibet kvāthayitvā sa-śārivam ।
atha-vā tri-phalā-musta-bhūnimba-kaṭu-rohiṇīḥ ।।

śārivādiṃ paṭolādiṃ padmakādiṃ tathā gaṇam ।
ghṛtāny ebhiś ca siddhāni pitta-ghnaṃ ca virecanam ।।

śītāṃś cābhyaṅga-lepādīn yuñjyāc chleṣmātmake punaḥ ।
yaṣṭy-āhva-saindhava-yutaṃ kumāraṃ pāyayed ghṛtam ।।

sindhūttha-pippalī-mad vā piṣṭaiḥ kṣaudra-yutair atha ।
rāṭha-puṣpaiḥ stanau limpec chiśoś ca daśana-cchadau ।।

indhūttha-pippalī-madya- indhūttha-pippalī-mustā- indhūttha-pippalī-mūrvā- 
-piṣṭaiḥ kṣaudra-yutair atha
sukham evaṃ vamed bālaḥ tīkṣṇair dhātrīṃ tu vāmayet ।
athācarita-saṃsargī mustādiṃ kvathitaṃ pibet ।।

tad-vat tagara-pṛthvīkā-suradāru-kaliṅgakān ।
atha-vātiviṣā-musta-ṣaḍgranthā-pañca-kolakam ।।

-suradāru-kaliṅgakam -ṣaḍgranthā-pañca-kolakān
stanye tri-doṣa-maline dur-gandhy āmaṃ jalopamam ।
vibaddham acchaṃ vicchinnaṃ phenilaṃ copaveśyate ।।

śakṛn nānā-vyathā-varṇaṃ mūtraṃ pītaṃ sitaṃ ghanam ।
jvarā-rocaka-tṛṭ-chardi-śuṣkodgāra-vijṛmbhikāḥ ।।

aṅga-bhaṅgo aṅga-vikṣepaḥ kūjanaṃ vepathur bhramaḥ ।
ghrāṇākṣi-mukha-pākādyā jāyante anye api taṃ gadam ।।

vaṇanaṃ vepathur bhramaḥ
kṣīrālasakam ity āhur atyayaṃ cāti-dāruṇam ।
tatrāśu dhātrīṃ bālaṃ ca vamanenopapādayet ।।

vihitāyāṃ ca saṃsargyāṃ vacādiṃ yojayed gaṇam ।
niśādiṃ vātha-vā mādrī-pāṭhā-tiktā-ghanāmayān ।।

pāṭhā-śuṇṭhy-amṛtā-tikta-tiktā-devāhva-śārivāḥ ।
sa-musta-mūrvendrayavāḥ stanya-doṣa-harāḥ param ।।

anubandhe yathā-vyādhi pratikurvīta kāla-vit ।
dantodbhedaś ca rogāṇāṃ sarveṣām api kāraṇam ।।

viśeṣāj jvara-viḍ-bheda-kāsa-cchardi-śiro-rujām ।
abhiṣyandasya pothakyā visarpasya ca jāyate ।।

pṛṣṭha-bhaṅge biḍālānāṃ barhiṇāṃ ca śikhodbhave ।
dantodbhede ca bālānāṃ na hi kiñ-cin na dūyate ।।

antodbhave ca bālānāṃ
yathā-doṣaṃ yathā-rogaṃ yathodrekaṃ yathā-bhayam ।
vibhajya deśa-kālādīṃs tatra yojyaṃ bhiṣag-jitam ।।

athodrekaṃ yathā-balam athodrekaṃ yathā-vayaḥ 
yathodrekaṃ yathāśayam
ta eva doṣā dūṣyāś ca jvarādyā vyādhayaś ca yat ।
atas tad eva bhaiṣajyaṃ mātrā tv asya kanīyasī ।।

varādyā vyādhayaś ca te
saukumāryālpa-kāya-tvāt sarvānnān-upasevanāt ।
snigdhā eva sadā bālā ghṛta-kṣīra-niṣevaṇāt ।।

arvānnān-upasevanaiḥ
sadyas tān vamanaṃ tasmāt pāyayen mati-mān mṛdu ।
stanyasya tṛptaṃ vamayet kṣīra-kṣīrānna-sevinam ।।

pīta-vantaṃ tanuṃ peyām annādaṃ ghṛta-saṃyutām ।
vastiṃ sādhye virekeṇa marśena pratimarśanam ।।

yuñjyād virecanādīṃs tu dhātryā eva yathoditān ।
mūrvā-vyoṣa-varā-kola-jambū-tvag-dāru-sarṣapāḥ ।।

uñjyād virecanādīṃś ca ūrvā-vyoṣa-vacā-kola- 
mūrvā-vyoṣa-varāṅkolla-
sa-pāṭhā madhunā līḍhāḥ stanya-doṣa-harāḥ param ।
danta-pālīṃ sa-madhunā cūrṇena pratisārayet ।।

tanya-doṣa-nibarhaṇāḥ
pippalyā dhātakī-puṣpa-dhātrī-phala-kṛtena vā ।
lāva-tittiri-vallūra-rajaḥ puṣpa-rasa-drutam ।।

-dhātrī-phala-rasena vā -rajaḥ puṣpa-rasa-plutam -rajaḥ 
puṣpa-rasāplutam
drutaṃ karoti bālānāṃ danta-kesara-van mukham ।
vacā-dvi-bṛhatī-pāṭhā-kaṭukātiviṣā-ghanaiḥ ।।

madhuraiś ca ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ siddhaṃ daśana-janmani ।
rajanī-dāru-sarala-śreyasī-bṛhatī-dvayam ।।

ajanī-dāru-saralāḥ śreyasī-bṛhatī-dvayam
pṛśniparṇī śatāhvā ca līḍhaṃ mākṣika-sarpiṣā ।
grahaṇī-dīpanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mārutasyānulomanam ।।

atīsāra-jvara-śvāsa-kāmalā-pāṇḍu-kāsa-nut ।
bālasya sarva-rogeṣu pūjitaṃ bala-varṇa-dam ।।

-kāmalā-pāṇḍu-roga-nut
samaṅgā-dhātakī-lodhra-kuṭannaṭa-balā-dvayaiḥ ।
mahā-sahā-kṣudra-sahā-mudga-bilva-śalāṭubhiḥ ।।

-kuṭannaṭa-balāhvayaiḥ -kuṭannaṭa-vaṭāhvayaiḥ
sa-kārpāsī-phalais toye sādhitaiḥ sādhitaṃ ghṛtam ।
kṣīra-mastu-yutaṃ hanti śīghraṃ dantodbhavodbhavān ।।

vividhān āmayān etad vṛddha-kāśyapa-nirmitam ।
dantodbhaveṣu rogeṣu na bālam atiyantrayet ।।

antodbhedottha-rogeṣu
svayam apy upaśāmyanti jāta-dantasya yad-gadāḥ ।
aty-ahaḥ-svapna-śītāmbu-ślaiṣmika-stanya-sevinaḥ ।।

-ślaiṣmika-stanya-pāyinaḥ
śiśoḥ kaphena ruddheṣu srotaḥsu rasa-vāhiṣu ।
a-rocakaḥ pratiśyāyo jvaraḥ kāsaś ca jāyate ।।

kumāraḥ śuṣyati tataḥ snigdha-śukla-mukhekṣaṇaḥ ।
saindhava-vyoṣa-śārṅgaṣṭā-pāṭhā-giri-kadambakān ।।

-pāṭhā-giri-kadambakam
śuṣyato madhu-sarpirbhyām a-rucy-ādiṣu yojayet ।
aśoka-rohiṇī-yuktaṃ pañca-kolaṃ ca cūrṇitam ।।

badarī-dhātakī-dhātrī-cūrṇaṃ vā sarpiṣā drutam ।
sthirā-vacā-dvi-bṛhatī-kākolī-pippalī-nataiḥ ।।

-cūrṇaṃ vā sarpiṣāplutam
niculotpala-varṣābhū-bhārgī-mustaiś ca kārṣikaiḥ ।
siddhaṃ prasthārdham ājyasya srotasāṃ śodhanaṃ param ।।

siṃhy-aśvagandhā-surasā-kaṇā-garbhaṃ ca tad-guṇam ।
yaṣṭy-āhva-pippalī-lodhra-padmakotpala-candanaiḥ ।।

tālīśa-śārivābhyāṃ ca sādhitaṃ śoṣa-jid ghṛtam ।
śṛṅgī-madhūlikā-bhārgī-pippalī-devadārubhiḥ ।।

aśvagandhā-dvi-kākolī-rāsnarṣabhaka-jīvakaiḥ ।
śūrpaparṇī-viḍaṅgaiś ca kalkitaiḥ sādhitaṃ ghṛtam ।।

śaśottamāṅga-niryūhe śuṣyataḥ puṣṭi-kṛt param ।
vacā-vayaḥsthā-tagara-kāyasthā-corakaiḥ śṛtam ।।

basta-mūtra-surābhyāṃ ca tailam abhyañjane hitam ।
lākṣā-rasa-samaṃ taila-prasthaṃ mastu catur-guṇam ।।

ailān mastu catur-guṇam ākṣā-rasa-samaṃ tailaṃ 
prasthaṃ mastu catur-guṇam
aśvagandhā-niśā-dāru-kauntī-kuṣṭhābda-candanaiḥ ।
sa-mūrvā-rohiṇī-rāsnā-śatāhvā-madhukaiḥ samaiḥ ।।

siddhaṃ lākṣādikaṃ nāma tailam abhyañjanād idam ।
balyaṃ jvara-kṣayonmāda-śvāsāpasmāra-vāta-nut ।।

yakṣa-rākṣasa-bhūta-ghnaṃ garbhiṇīnāṃ ca śasyate ।
madhunātiviṣā-śṛṅgī-pippalīr lehayec chiśum ।।

ekāṃ vātiviṣāṃ kāsa-jvara-cchardir-upadrutam ।
pītaṃ pītaṃ vamati yaḥ stanyaṃ taṃ madhu-sarpiṣā ।।

-jvara-cchardibhir arditam ītaṃ pītaṃ ca vamati aḥ 
stanyaṃ madhu-sarpiṣā
dvi-vārtākī-phala-rasaṃ pañca-kolaṃ ca lehayet ।
pippalī-pañca-lavaṇaṃ kṛmijit-pāribhadrakam ।।

ippalī-pañca-lavaṇa- -kṛmijit-pāribhadrakam iḍaṅgaṃ 
pāribhadrakam
tad-val lihyāt tathā vyoṣaṃ maṣīṃ vā roma-carmaṇām ।
lābhataḥ śalyaka-śvāvid-godharkṣa-śikhi-janmanām ।।

khadirārjuna-tālīśa-kuṣṭha-candana-je rase ।
sa-kṣīraṃ sādhitaṃ sarpir vamathuṃ viniyacchati ।।

hanu-mūla-gato vāyur danta-deśāsthi-go-caraḥ ।
yadā śiśoḥ prakupito nottiṣṭhanti tadā dvi-jāḥ ।।

hanu-mūlāśrito vāyur danta-deśān viśoṣayet 
danta-deśān viśodhayet
rūkṣāśino vātikasya cālayaty anilaḥ sirāḥ ।
hanv-āśrayāḥ prasuptasya dantaiḥ śabdaṃ karoty ataḥ ।।

sa-danto jāyate yas tu dantāḥ prāg yasya cottarāḥ ।
kurvīta tasminn utpāte śāntiṃ taṃ ca dvi-jātaye ।।

śāntikaṃ ca dvi-jātaye
dadyāt sa-dakṣiṇaṃ bālaṃ naigameṣaṃ ca pūjayet ।
tālu-māṃse kaphaḥ kruddhaḥ kurute tālu-kaṇṭakam ।।

ainikeśaṃ ca pūjayet
tena tālu-pradeśasya nimna-tā mūrdhni jāyate ।
tālu-pātaḥ stana-dveṣaḥ kṛcchrāt pānaṃ śakṛd-dravam ।।

tṛḍ-āsya-kaṇḍv-akṣi-rujā grīvā-dur-dhara-tā vamiḥ ।
tatrotkṣipya yava-kṣāra-kṣaudrābhyāṃ pratisārayet ।।

tālu tad-vat kaṇā-śuṇṭhī-go-śakṛd-rasa-saindhavaiḥ ।
śṛṅgavera-niśā-bhṛṅgaṃ kalkitaṃ vaṭa-pallavaiḥ ।।

baddhvā go-śakṛtā liptam kukūle svedayet tataḥ ।
rasena limpet tālv-āsyaṃ netre ca pariṣecayet ।।

harītakī-vacā-kuṣṭha-kalkaṃ mākṣika-saṃyutam ।
pītvā kumāraḥ stanyena mucyate tālu-kaṇṭakāt ।।

malopalepāt svedād vā gude rakta-kaphodbhavaḥ ।
tāmro vraṇo antaḥ kaṇḍū-mān jāyate bhūry-upadravaḥ ।।

ke-cit taṃ mātṛkā-doṣaṃ vadanty anye ahi-pūtanam ।
pṛṣṭhārur guda-kuṭṭaṃ ca ke-cic ca tam a-nāmikam ।।

e-cic ca tam a-nāmakam adanty anye api pūtanam adanty anye tu pūtanam c vadanty anye hi pūtanam ṛṣṭhārur guda-kaṇḍūṃ ca ṛṣṭhārur guda-kiṭṭaṃ ca 
ṛṣṭhārur guda-kuṣṭhaṃ ca
tatra dhātryāḥ payaḥ śodhyaṃ pitta-śleṣma-harauṣadhaiḥ ।
śṛta-śītaṃ ca śītāmbu-yuktam antara-pānakam ।।

ita-śītaṃ ca śītāmbu-
sa-kṣaudra-tārkṣya-śailena vraṇaṃ tena ca lepayet ।
tri-phalā-badarī-plakṣa-tvak-kvātha-pariṣecitam ।।

kāsīsa-rocanā-tuttha-manohvāla-rasāñjanaiḥ ।
lepayed amla-piṣṭair vā cūrṇitair vāvacūrṇayet ।।

su-ślakṣṇair atha-vā yaṣṭī-śaṅkha-sauvīrakāñjanaiḥ ।
śārivā-śaṅkhanābhibhyām asanasya tvacātha-vā ।।

rāga-kaṇḍūtkaṭe kuryād rakta-srāvaṃ jalaukasā ।
sarvaṃ ca pitta-vraṇa-jic chasyate guda-kuṭṭake ।।

hasyate guda-kiṭṭake
pāṭhā-vella-dvi-rajanī-musta-bhārgī-punarnavaiḥ ।
sa-bilva-try-ūṣaṇaiḥ sarpiḥ vṛścikālī-yutaiḥ śṛtam ।।
lihāno mātrayā rogair mucyate mṛttikodbhavaiḥ ।।vyādher yady asya bhaiṣajyaṃ stanas tena pralepitaḥ ।।sthito muhūrtaṃ dhauto anu pītas taṃ taṃ jayed gadam ।।
ītas tat taṃ jayed gadam

uttarasthāna
purā guhasya rakṣārthaṃ nirmitāḥ śūla-pāṇinā ।
manuṣya-vigrahāḥ pañca sapta strī-vigrahā grahāḥ ।।

skando viśākho meṣākhyaḥ śva-grahaḥ pitṛ-saṃjñitaḥ ।
śakuniḥ pūtanā śīta-pūtanā-dṛṣṭi-pūtanā ।।

kando viśākho meṣāsyaḥ
mukha-maṇḍitikā tad-vad revatī śuṣka-revatī ।
teṣāṃ grahīṣyatāṃ rūpaṃ pratataṃ rodanaṃ jvaraḥ ।।

ukha-maṇḍanikā tad-vad ukha-maṇḍinikā tad-vad
sāmānyaṃ rūpam uttrāsa-jṛmbhā-bhrū-kṣepa-dīna-tāḥ ।
phena-srāvordhva-dṛṣṭy-oṣṭha-danta-daṃśa-prajāgarāḥ ।।

-jṛmbhā-bhrūtkṣepa-dīna-tāḥ
rodanaṃ kūjanaṃ stanya-vidveṣaḥ svara-vaikṛtam ।
nakhair a-kasmāt paritaḥ sva-dhātry-aṅga-vilekhanam ।।

tatraika-nayana-srāvī śiro vikṣipate muhuḥ ।
hataika-pakṣaḥ stabdhāṅgaḥ sa-svedo nata-kandharaḥ ।।

śiro vikṣepate muhuḥ śiro vikṣipyate muhuḥ
danta-khādī stana-dveṣī trasyan roditi vi-svaram ।
vakra-vaktro vaman lālāṃ bhṛśam ūrdhvaṃ nirīkṣate ।।

rasan roditi vi-svaram akra-vaktro vamel lālāṃ
vasāsṛg-gandhir udvigno baddha-muṣṭi-śakṛc chiśuḥ ।
calitaikākṣi-gaṇḍa-bhrūḥ saṃraktobhaya-locanaḥ ।।

skandārtas tena vaikalyaṃ maraṇaṃ vā bhaved dhruvam ।
saṃjñā-nāśo muhuḥ keśa-luñcanaṃ kandharā-natiḥ ।।

araṇaṃ vā bhaved drutam aṃjñā-nāśo bhavet keśa-
vinamya jṛmbhamāṇasya śakṛn-mūtra-pravartanam ।
phenodvamanam ūrdhvekṣā hasta-bhrū-pāda-nartanam ।।

stana-sva-jihvā-saṃdaṃśa-saṃrambha-jvara-jāgarāḥ ।
pūya-śoṇita-gandhaś ca skandāpasmāra-lakṣaṇam ।।

ādhmānaṃ pāṇi-pādasya spandanaṃ phena-nirvamaḥ ।
tṛṇ-muṣṭi-bandhātīsāra-svara-dainya-vi-varṇa-tāḥ ।।

ādhmānaṃ pāṇi-pādāsya- -spandanaṃ phena-nirvamaḥ pandanaṃ phena-nirgamaḥ 
pandanaṃ hananaṃ bhramaḥ
kūjanaṃ stananaṃ chardiḥ kāsa-hidhmā-prajāgarāḥ ।
oṣṭha-daṃśāṅga-saṃkoca-stambha-bastābha-gandha-tāḥ ।।

ūjanaṃ śvasanaṃ chardiḥ ūjanaṃ stambhanaṃ chardiḥ 
kūjanaṃ svananaṃ chardiḥ
ūrdhvaṃ nirīkṣya hasanaṃ madhye vinamanaṃ jvaraḥ ।
mūrchaika-netra-śophaś ca naigameṣa-grahākṛtiḥ ।।

kampo hṛṣita-roma-tvaṃ svedaś cakṣur-nimīlanam ।
bahir-āyāmanaṃ jihvā-daṃśo antaḥ-kaṇṭha-kūjanam ।।

ampo harṣita-roma-tvaṃ
dhāvanaṃ viṭ-sa-gandha-tvaṃ krośanaṃ ca śva-vac chuni ।
roma-harṣo muhus trāsaḥ sahasā rodanaṃ jvaraḥ ।।

rośanaṃ śvāna-vac chuni oma-harṣo muhuḥ śvāsaḥ
kāsātīsāra-vamathu-jṛmbhā-tṛṭ-śava-gandha-tāḥ ।
aṅgeṣv ākṣepa-vikṣepa-śoṣa-stambha-vi-varṇa-tāḥ ।।

muṣṭi-bandhaḥ srutiś cākṣṇor bālasya syuḥ pitṛ-grahe ।
srastāṅga-tvam atīsāro jihvā-tālu-gale vraṇāḥ ।।

sphoṭāḥ sa-dāha-ruk-pākāḥ saṃdhiṣu syuḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
niśy ahni pravilīyante pāko vaktre gude api vā ।।

bhayaṃ śakuni-gandha-tvaṃ jvaraś ca śakuni-grahe ।
pūtanāyāṃ vamiḥ kampas tandrā rātrau prajāgaraḥ ।।

hidhmādhmānaṃ śakṛd-bhedaḥ pipāsā mūtra-nigrahaḥ ।
srasta-hṛṣṭāṅga-roma-tvaṃ kāka-vat pūti-gandhi-tā ।।

śīta-pūtanayā kampo rodanaṃ tiryag-īkṣaṇam ।
tṛṣṇāntra-kūjo atīsāro vasā-vad visra-gandha-tā ।।

pārśvasyaikasya śīta-tvam uṣṇa-tvam aparasya ca ।
andha-pūtanayā chardir jvaraḥ kāso alpa-nidra-tā ।।

varaḥ kāso alpa-vahni-tā
varcaso bheda-vaivarṇya-daurgandhyāny aṅga-śoṣaṇam ।
dṛṣṭeḥ sādāti-ruk-kaṇḍū-pothakī-janma-śūna-tāḥ ।।

ṛṣṭi-prasādo ruk-kaṇḍū- ṛṣṭi-sādo akṣi-ruk-kaṇḍū- ṛṣṭi-sādo ati-ruk kaṇḍūḥ ṛṣṭi-sādo ati-ruk-kaṇḍū- ṛṣṭeḥ sādo akṣi-ruk-kaṇḍū- othakī-janma śūna-tā 
-pothakī-janma śūna-tā -pothakī-janma śūnya-tā
hidhmodvega-stana-dveṣa-vaivarṇya-svara-tīkṣṇa-tāḥ ।
vepathur matsya-gandha-tvam atha-vā sāmla-gandha-tā ।।

-vaivarṇyaṃ svara-tīkṣṇa-tā amathur matsya-gandha-tvam
mukha-maṇḍitayā pāṇi-pādāsya-ramaṇīya-tā ।
sirābhir asitābhābhir ācitodara-tā jvaraḥ ।।

ukha-maṇḍikayā pāṇi- -pādasya ramaṇīya-tā
a-rocako aṅga-glapanaṃ go-mūtra-sama-gandha-tā ।
revatyāṃ śyāva-nīla-tvaṃ karṇa-nāsākṣi-mardanam ।।

evatyā śyāva-nīla-tvaṃ
kāsa-hidhmākṣi-vikṣepa-vakra-vaktra-tva-rakta-tāḥ ।
basta-gandho jvaraḥ śoṣaḥ purīṣaṃ haritaṃ dravam ।।

jāyate śuṣka-revatyāṃ kramāt sarvāṅga-saṃkṣayaḥ ।
keśa-śāto anna-vidveṣaḥ svara-dainyaṃ vi-varṇa-tā ।।

āyate śuṣka-revatyā nānā-varṇa-purīṣa-tvam udare granthayaḥ sirāḥ ।।

rodanaṃ gṛdhra-gandha-tvaṃ dīrgha-kālānuvartanam ।
udare granthayo vṛttā yasya nānā-vidhaṃ śakṛt ।।

jihvāyā nimna-tā madhye śyāvaṃ tālu ca taṃ tyajet ।
bhuñjāno annaṃ bahu-vidhaṃ yo bālaḥ parihīyate ।।

ihvāyāṃ nimna-tā madhye
tṛṣṇā-gṛhītaḥ kṣāmākṣo hanti taṃ śuṣka-revatī ।
hiṃsā-raty-arcanākāṅkṣā graha-grahaṇa-kāraṇam ।।

tatra hiṃsātmake bālo mahān vā sruta-nāsikaḥ ।
kṣata-jihvaḥ kvaṇed bāḍham a-sukhī sāśru-locanaḥ ।।

ṣata-jihvaḥ kvaṇan bāḍham ṣata-jihvaḥ kvaṇed gāḍham ṣata-jihvo vamed bāḍham 
-sukhī sāsra-locanaḥ
dur-varṇo hīna-vacanaḥ pūti-gandhiś ca jāyate ।
kṣāmo mūtra-purīṣaṃ svaṃ mṛdnāti na jugupsate ।।

ūti-gandhis tu jāyate ṛhṇāti na jugupsate
hastau codyamya saṃrabdho hanty ātmānaṃ tathā param ।
tad-vac ca śastra-kāṣṭhādyair agniṃ vā dīptam āviśet ।।

astau codyamya saṃkruddho
apsu majjet patet kūpe kuryād anyac ca tad-vidham ।
tṛḍ-dāha-mohān pūyasya cchardanaṃ ca pravartayet ।।

ṛḍ-dāha-mohāḥ pūyasya
raktaṃ ca sarva-mārgebhyo riṣṭotpattiṃ ca taṃ tyajet ।
rahaḥ-strī-rati-saṃlāpa-gandha-srag-bhūṣaṇa-priyaḥ ।।

iṣṭotpattiś ca taṃ tyajet
hṛṣṭaḥ śāntaś ca duḥ-sādhyo rati-kāmena pīḍitaḥ ।
dīnaḥ parimṛśan vaktraṃ śuṣkauṣṭha-gala-tālukaḥ ।।

īnaḥ parimṛśed vaktraṃ
śaṅkitaṃ vīkṣate rauti dhyāyaty āyāti dīna-tām ।
annam annābhilāṣe api dattaṃ nāti bubhukṣate ।।

gṛhītaṃ bali-kāmena taṃ vidyāt sukha-sādhanam ।
hantu-kāmaṃ jayed dhomaiḥ siddha-mantra-pravartitaiḥ ।।

ṛhītaṃ maha-kāmena
itarau tu yathā-kāmaṃ rati-baly-ādi-dānataḥ ।
atha sādhya-grahaṃ bālaṃ vivikte śaraṇe sthitam ।।

trir ahnaḥ sikta-saṃmṛṣṭe sadā saṃnihitānale ।
vikīrṇa-bhūti-kusuma-pattra-bījānna-sarṣape ।।

rir ahnaṃ sikta-saṃmṛṣṭe rir ahnaḥ sikta-saṃsṛṣṭe rir ahni sikta-saṃmṛṣṭe 
rir ahni sikta-saṃsṛṣṭe ikīrṇa-bhūri-kusuma-
rakṣo-ghna-taila-jvalita-pradīpa-hata-pāpmani ।
vyavāya-madya-piśita-nivṛtta-paricārake ।।

-pradīpe hata-pāpmani
purāṇa-sarpiṣābhyaktaṃ pariṣiktaṃ sukhāmbunā ।
sādhitena balā-nimba-vaijayantī-nṛpadrumaiḥ ।।

pāribhadraka-kaṭvaṅga-jambū-varuṇa-kaṭtṛṇaiḥ ।
kapotavaṅkāpāmārga-pāṭalā-madhu-śigrubhiḥ ।।

-pāṭalī-madhuśigrubhiḥ -mālatī-madhuśigrubhiḥ
kākajaṅghā-mahāśvetā-kapittha-kṣīri-pādapaiḥ ।
sa-kadamba-karañjaiś ca dhūpaṃ snātasya cācaret ।।

-kapittha-kṣīra-pādapaiḥ
dvīpi-vyāghrāhi-siṃharkṣa-carmabhir ghṛta-miśritaiḥ ।
pūti-daśāṅga-siddhārtha-vacā-bhallāta-dīpyakaiḥ ।।

ūti-daśāṅgī-siddhārtha-
sa-kuṣṭhaiḥ sa-ghṛtair dhūpaḥ sarva-graha-vimokṣaṇaḥ ।
sarṣapā nimba-pattrāṇi mūlam aśvakhurā vacā ।।

a-kuṣṭhaiḥ sādhito dhūpaḥ ūtram aśvakhurā vacā 
mūlam aśvakhuraṃ vacā
bhūrja-pattraṃ ghṛtaṃ dhūpaḥ sarva-graha-nivāraṇaḥ ।
anantāmrāsthi-tagaraṃ maricaṃ madhuro gaṇaḥ ।।

arva-graha-nibarhaṇaḥ nantāmrāsthi-tagara- -maricaṃ 
madhuro gaṇaḥ
śṛgālavinnā mustā ca kalkitais tair ghṛtaṃ pacet ।
daśa-mūla-rasa-kṣīra-yuktaṃ tad graha-jit param ।।

rāsnā-dvy-aṃśumatī-vṛddha-pañca-mūla-balā-ghanāt ।
kvāthe sarpiḥ pacet piṣṭaiḥ śārivā-vyoṣa-citrakaiḥ ।।

āsnā-dvy-aṃśumatī-pattra- āsnā-dvy-aṃśumatī-lodhra- 
-pañca-mūla-vacā-ghanāt
pāṭhā-viḍaṅga-madhuka-payasyā-hiṅgu-dārubhiḥ ।
sa-granthikaiḥ sendrayavaiḥ śiśos tat satataṃ hitam ।।

śiśos tu satataṃ hitam
sarva-roga-graha-haraṃ dīpanaṃ bala-varṇa-dam ।
śārivā-surabhi-brāhmī-śaṅkhinī-kuṣṭha-sarṣapaiḥ ।।

īpanaṃ bala-vardhanam -śaṅkhinī-kṛṣṇa-sarṣapaiḥ
