vacāśvagandhā-surasa-yuktaiḥ sarpir vipācayet ।
tan nāśayed grahān sarvān pānenābhyañjanena ca ।।

acāśvagandhā-surasā-
go-śṛṅga-carma-vālāhi-nirmokaṃ vṛṣa-daṃśa-viṭ ।
nimba-pattrājya-kaṭukā-madanaṃ bṛhatī-dvayam ।।

o-śṛṅga-carma-vālāsthi- o-śṛṅga-roma-vālāhi-
kārpāsāsthi-yava-cchāga-roma-devāhva-sarṣapam ।
mayūra-pattra-śrīvāsaṃ tuṣa-keśaṃ sa-rāmaṭham ।।

ārpāsāsthi-yava-vacā- ārpāsāsthi-vacā-bilva- ārpāsāsthi-vacā-lodhra- ayūra-piccha-śrīvāsa- ayūra-piccha-śrīvāsaṃ -lodhra-devāhva-sarṣapam -devāhvaṃ yava-sarṣapam ayūra-pattra-śrīvāsa- 
-nara-keśaṃ sa-rāmaṭham
mṛd-bhāṇḍe basta-mūtreṇa bhāvitaṃ ślakṣṇa-cūrṇitam ।
dhūpanaṃ ca hitaṃ sarva-bhūteṣu viṣama-jvare ।।

hūpanārthaṃ hitaṃ sarva-
ghṛtāni bhūta-vidyāyāṃ vakṣyante yāni tāni ca ।
yuñjyāt tathā baliṃ homaṃ snapanaṃ mantra-tantra-vit ।।

pūti-karañja-tvak-pattraṃ kṣīribhyo barbarād api ।
tumbī-viśālāraluka-śamī-bilva-kapitthataḥ ।।

ūti-karañja-tvak-pattra- ūti-karañjāt tvak-pattraṃ -kṣīribhyo vedarād api -mūlebhyo barbarād api -mūlebhyo vardharād api 
-śamī-bilva-kapitthakam
utkvāthya toyaṃ tad rātrau bālānāṃ snapanaṃ śivam ।
anubandhān yathā-kṛcchraṃ grahāpāye apy upadravān ।।

raha-vyāpady upadravān bālāmaya-niṣedhokta-bheṣajaiḥ samupācaret ।।

ū̆-bhaiṣajyaiḥ samupācaret

uttarasthāna
lakṣayej jñāna-vijñāna-vāk-ceṣṭā-bala-pauruṣam ।
puruṣe a-pauruṣaṃ yatra tatra bhūta-grahaṃ vadet ।।

bhūtasya rūpa-prakṛti-bhāṣā-gaty-ādi-ceṣṭitaiḥ ।
yasyānukāraṃ kurute tenāviṣṭaṃ tam ādiśet ।।

so aṣṭā-daśa-vidho deva-dānavādi-vibhedataḥ ।
hetus tad-anuṣaktau tu sadyaḥ pūrva-kṛto atha-vā ।।

adyaḥ pūrvaṃ kṛto atha-vā
prajñāparādhaḥ su-tarāṃ tena kāmādi-janmanā ।
lupta-dharma-vratācāraḥ pūjyān apy ativartate ।।

ūjyānām ativartanaiḥ
taṃ tathā bhinna-maryādaṃ pāpam ātmopaghātinam ।
devādayo apy anughnanti grahāś chidra-prahāriṇaḥ ।।

chidraṃ pāpa-kriyārambhaḥ pāko an-iṣṭasya karmaṇaḥ ।
ekasya śūnye avasthānaṃ śmaśānādiṣu vā niśi ।।

dig-vāsas-tvaṃ guror nindā rater a-vidhi-sevanam ।
a-śucer devatārcādi para-sūtaka-saṃkaraḥ ।।

-śucer devatārāddhiḥ ara-sūtaka-saṃkarāt
homa-mantra-balījyānāṃ vi-guṇaṃ parikarma ca ।
samāsād dina-caryādi-proktācāra-vyatikramaḥ ।।

-proktānāṃ ca viparyayaḥ
gṛhṇanti śukla-pratipat-trayo-daśyoḥ surā naram ।
śukla-trayo-daśī-kṛṣṇa-dvā-daśyor dānavā grahāḥ ।।

-dvā-daśyor dānava-grahāḥ
gandharvās tu catur-daśyāṃ dvā-daśyāṃ coragāḥ punaḥ ।
pañcamyāṃ śukla-saptamy-ekā-daśyos tu dhaneśvarāḥ ।।

añcamyāṃ śukla-saptamyām kā-daśyāṃ dhaneśvarāḥ
śuklāṣṭa-pañcamī-paurṇamāsīṣu brahma-rākṣasāḥ ।
kṛṣṇe rakṣaḥ-piśācādyā nava-dvā-daśa-parvasu ।।

śuklāṣṭa-pañcamī-pūrṇa- -māsīṣu brahma-rākṣasāḥ
daśāmāvāsyayor aṣṭa-navamyoḥ pitaro apare ।
guru-vṛddhādayaḥ prāyaḥ kālaṃ saṃdhyāsu lakṣayet ।।

arśāmāvāsyayor aṣṭa- aśāmāvāsyayoḥ ṣaṣṭhī-
phulla-padmopama-mukhaṃ saumya-dṛṣṭim a-kopanam ।
alpa-vāk-sveda-viṇ-mūtraṃ bhojanān-abhilāṣiṇam ।।

v-alpa-vāk-sveda-viṇ-mūtraṃ
deva-dvi-jāti-paramaṃ śuciṃ saṃskṛta-vādinam ।
mīlayantaṃ cirān netre surabhiṃ vara-dāyinam ।।

śukla-mālyāmbara-saric-chailocca-bhavana-priyam ।
a-nidram a-pradhṛṣyaṃ ca vidyād deva-vaśī-kṛtam ।।

śukla-mālyāmbara-dharaṃ śailocca-bhavana-priyam
jihma-dṛṣṭiṃ dur-ātmānaṃ guru-deva-dvi-ja-dviṣam ।
nir-bhayaṃ māninaṃ śūraṃ krodhanaṃ vyavasāyinam ।।

ir-bhayaṃ māninaṃ krūraṃ
rudraḥ skando viśākho aham indro aham iti vādinam ।
surā-māṃsa-ruciṃ vidyād daitya-graha-gṛhītakam ।।

udraḥ skandaḥ piśāco aham adya-māṃsa-ruciṃ vidyād 
daitya-graha-vaśī-kṛtam
sv-ācāraṃ surabhiṃ hṛṣṭaṃ gīta-nartana-kāriṇam ।
snānodyāna-ruciṃ rakta-vastra-mālyānulepanam ।।

v-ācāra-surabhi-śiṣṭa- ve-caraṃ surabhiṃ hṛṣṭaṃ -gīta-nartana-kāriṇam 
nānodyāna-rataṃ rakta-
śṛṅgāra-līlābhirataṃ gandharvādhyuṣitaṃ vadet ।
raktākṣaṃ krodhanaṃ stabdha-dṛṣṭiṃ vakra-gatiṃ calam ।।

śṛṅgāra-mālyābhirataṃ śṛṅgāra-līlābhihitaṃ
śvasantam a-niśaṃ jihvā-lolinaṃ sṛkkiṇī-liham ।
priya-dugdha-guḍa-snānam adho-vadana-śāyinam ।।

uragādhiṣṭhitaṃ vidyāt trasyantaṃ cātapa-trataḥ ।
vipluta-trasta-raktākṣaṃ śubha-gandhaṃ su-tejasam ।।

priya-nṛtya-kathā-gīta-snāna-mālyānulepanam ।
matsya-māṃsa-ruciṃ hṛṣṭaṃ tuṣṭaṃ balinam a-vyatham ।।

riya-narta-kathā-gīta- atsya-māṃsa-ruciṃ hṛṣṭa- -tuṣṭaṃ balinam a-vyatham 
uṣṭaṃ balinam a-vyayam
calitāgra-karaṃ kasmai kiṃ dadāmīti vādinam ।
rahasya-bhāṣiṇaṃ vaidya-dvi-jāti-paribhāvinam ।।

-dvi-jāti-parivādinam
alpa-roṣaṃ druta-gatiṃ vidyād yakṣa-gṛhītakam ।
hāsya-nṛtya-priyaṃ raudra-ceṣṭaṃ chidra-prahāriṇam ।।

lpa-roṣaṃ hṛta-gatiṃ āsya-nṛtta-priyaṃ raudra- 
hāsya-nṛtya-karaṃ raudra-
ākrośinaṃ śīghra-gatiṃ deva-dvi-ja-bhiṣag-dviṣam ।
ātmānaṃ kāṣṭha-śastrādyair ghnantaṃ bhoḥ-śabda-vādinam ।।

hnantaṃ go-śabda-vādinam
śāstra-veda-paṭhaṃ vidyād gṛhītaṃ brahma-rākṣasaiḥ ।
sa-krodha-dṛṣṭiṃ bhrū-kuṭīm udvahantaṃ sa-saṃbhramaṃ ।।

ṛhītaṃ brahma-rākṣasā
praharantaṃ pradhāvantaṃ śabdantaṃ bhairavānanam ।
annād vināpi balinaṃ naṣṭa-nidraṃ niśā-caram ।।

udantaṃ bhairavānanam
nir-lajjam a-śuciṃ śūraṃ krūraṃ paruṣa-bhāṣiṇam ।
roṣaṇaṃ rakta-mālya-strī-rakta-madyāmiṣa-priyam ।।

-megha-madyāmiṣa-priyam
dṛṣṭvā ca raktaṃ māṃsaṃ vālihānaṃ daśana-cchadau ।
hasantam anna-kāle ca rākṣasādhiṣṭhitaṃ vadet ।।

ṛṣṭvā ca rakta-māṃsāni ihānaṃ daśana-cchadau
a-svastha-cittaṃ naika-tra tiṣṭhantaṃ paridhāvinam ।
ucchiṣṭa-nṛtya-gandharva-hāsa-madyāmiṣa-priyam ।।

nirbhartsanād dīna-mukhaṃ rudantam a-nimittataḥ ।
nakhair likhantam ātmānaṃ rūkṣa-dhvasta-vapuḥ-svaram ।।

āvedayantam duḥkhādi saṃbaddhā-baddha-bhāṣiṇam ।
naṣṭa-smṛtiṃ śūnya-ratiṃ lolaṃ nagnaṃ malīmasam ।।

āvedayantam duḥkhāni
rathyā-caila-parīdhānaṃ tṛṇa-mālā-vibhūṣaṇam ।
ārohantaṃ ca kāṣṭhāśvaṃ tathā saṃkara-kūṭakam ।।

ārohantaṃ ca kāṣṭhāśma- -rāśiṃ saṃkara-kūṭakam athā 
saṃkāra-kūṭakam
bahv-āśinaṃ piśācena vijānīyād adhiṣṭhitam ।
pretākṛti-kriyā-gandhaṃ bhītam āhāra-vidviṣam ।।

hīrum āhāra-vidviṣam
tṛṇa-cchidaṃ ca pretena gṛhītaṃ naram ādiśet ।
bahu-pralāpaṃ kṛṣṇāsyaṃ pravilambita-yāyinam ।।

śūna-pralamba-vṛṣaṇaṃ kūṣmāṇḍādhiṣṭhitaṃ vadet ।
gṛhītvā kāṣṭha-loṣṭādi bhramantaṃ cīra-vāsasam ।।

ṛhītvā kāṣṭha-lohādi
nagnaṃ dhāvantam uttrasta-dṛṣṭiṃ tṛṇa-vibhūṣaṇam ।
śmaśāna-śūnyāyatana-rathyaika-druma-sevinam ।।

tilānna-madya-māṃseṣu satataṃ sakta-locanaṃ ।
niṣādādhiṣṭhitaṃ vidyād vadantaṃ paruṣāṇi ca ।।

aṃsaktaṃ rakta-locanam atataṃ rakta-locanam a-raktaṃ rakta-locanam 
arkoṭādhiṣṭhitaṃ vindyād
yācantam udakaṃ cānnaṃ trasta-lohita-locanam ।
ugra-vākyaṃ ca jānīyān naram aukiraṇārditam ।।

hāvantam udakaṃ nānnaṃ ācantam udakaṃ nānnaṃ ācantam udakānnaṃ ca akta-vitrasta-locanam aram autkiraṇārditam araṃ maukiraṇārditam 
aram uttaruṇārditam
gandha-mālya-ratiṃ satya-vādinaṃ parivepinam ।
bahu-nidraṃ ca jānīyād vetālena vaśī-kṛtam ।।

andha-mālya-rataṃ satya- andha-mālya-ruciṃ satya- -vādinaṃ parivedinam 
-vādinaṃ paridevinam aitālena vaśī-kṛtam
a-prasanna-dṛśaṃ dīna-vadanaṃ śuṣka-tālukam ।
calan-nayana-pakṣmāṇaṃ nidrāluṃ manda-pāvakam ।।

apasavya-parīdhānaṃ tila-māṃsa-guḍa-priyam ।
skhalad-vācaṃ ca jānīyāt pitṛ-graha-vaśī-kṛtam ।।

khalad-vācaṃ vijānīyāt
guru-vṛddharṣi-siddhābhiśāpa-cintānurūpataḥ ।
vyāhārāhāra-ceṣṭābhir yathā-svaṃ tad-grahaṃ vadet ।।

uru-vṛddharṣi-siddhānāṃ śāpa-cintānurūpataḥ ṃśāpa-cittānurūpataḥ śāpa-cittānurūpataḥ ihārāhāra-ceṣṭābhir athā-svaṃ 
taṃ grahaṃ vadet
kumāra-vṛndānugataṃ nagnam uddhata-mūrdha-jam ।
a-svastha-manasaṃ dairghya-kālikaṃ sa-grahaṃ tyajet ।।

uttarasthāna
bhūtaṃ jayed a-hiṃsecchaṃ japa-homa-bali-vrataiḥ ।
tapaḥ-śīla-samādhāna-dāna-jñāna-dayādibhiḥ ।।

hūtaṃ jayed a-hiṃsotthaṃ apaḥ-śīla-samādhyāna-
hiṅgu-vyoṣāla-nepālī-laśunārka-jaṭā-jaṭāḥ ।
ajalomī sa-golomī bhūtakeśī vacā latā ।।

-laśunārka-jaṭāmayāḥ hūtakeśī-vacā-latāḥ hūtakeśī vacā 
balā
kukkuṭī sarpagandhākhyā tilāḥ kāṇa-vikāṇike ।
vajraproktā vayaḥsthā ca śṛṅgī mohanavally api ।।

ilāḥ kāla-vikāṇike ilāḥ kāṇa-viṣāṇike athā kāṇa-vikāṇike 
ajraproktā vayaḥsthā vā
sroto-jāñjana-rakṣoghnaṃ rakṣo-ghnaṃ cānyad auṣadham ।
kharāśva-śvāvid-uṣṭrarkṣa-godhā-nakula-śalyakāt ।।

-godhā-nakula-matsyakāt
dvīpi-mārjāra-go-siṃha-vyāghra-sāmudra-sat-tvataḥ ।
carma-pitta-dvi-ja-nakhā varge asmin sādhayed ghṛtam ।।

purāṇam atha-vā tailaṃ navaṃ tat pāna-nasyayoḥ ।
abhyaṅge ca prayoktavyam eṣāṃ cūrṇaṃ ca dhūpane ।।

ebhiś ca guṭikāṃ yuñjyād añjane sāvapīḍane ।
pralepe kalkam eteṣāṃ kvāthaṃ ca pariṣecane ।।

ñjane sāvapīḍake
prayogo ayaṃ grahonmādān sāpasmārāñ chamaṃ nayet ।
gajāhvā-pippalī-mūla-vyoṣāmalaka-sarṣapān ।।

godhā-nakula-mārjāra-jhaṣa-pitta-prapeṣitān ।
nāvanābhyaṅga-sekeṣu vidadhīta grahāpahān ।।

-śaśa-pitta-prapeṣitān -ṛkṣa-pitta-prapeṣitān
siddhārthaka-vacā-hiṅgu-priyaṅgu-rajanī-dvayam ।
mañjiṣṭhā śveta-kaṭabhī varā śvetādrikarṇikā ।।

añjiṣṭhā-śveta-kaṭabhī- -varā-śvetādrikarṇikāḥ
nimbasya pattraṃ bījaṃ tu naktamāla-śirīṣayoḥ ।
surāhvaṃ try-ūṣaṇaṃ sarpir go-mūtre taiś catur-guṇe ।।

o-mūtre ca catur-guṇe
siddhaṃ siddhārthakaṃ nāma pāne nasye ca yojitam ।
grahān sarvān nihanty āśu viśeṣād āsurān grahān ।।

kṛtyā-lakṣmī-viṣonmāda-jvarāpasmāra-pāpma ca ।
ebhir evauṣadhair basta-vāriṇā kalpito a-gadaḥ ।।

-jvarāpasmāra-pāpma-nut
pāna-nasyāñjanālepa-snānodgharṣaṇa-yojitaḥ ।
guṇaiḥ pūrva-vad uddiṣṭo rāja-dvāre ca siddhi-kṛt ।।

a guṇaiḥ pūrva-vad diṣṭo
siddhārthaka-vyoṣa-vacāśvagandhā niśā-dvayaṃ hiṅgu-palāṇḍu-kandaḥ ।
bījaṃ karañjāt kusumaṃ śirīṣāt phalaṃ ca valkaṃ ca kapittha-vṛkṣāt ।।

iśā-dvayaṃ hiṅgu-palāṇḍu-kandam halaṃ ca kalkaś ca kapittha-vṛkṣāt halaṃ ca puṣpaṃ ca kapittha-vṛkṣāt halaṃ ca valkaś ca 
kapittha-vṛkṣāt
sa-māṇimanthaṃ sa-nataṃ sa-kuṣṭhaṃ śyoṇāka-mūlaṃ kiṇihī sitā ca ।
bastasya mūtreṇa su-bhāvitaṃ tat pittena gavyena guḍān vidadhyāt ।।

duṣṭa-vraṇonmāda-tamo-niśāndhān udbandhakān vāri-nimagna-dehān ।
digdhāhatān darpita-sarpa-daṣṭāṃs te sādhayanty añjana-nasya-lepaiḥ ।।

uṣṭa-vraṇonmāda-tamo-niśāndhyam dbaddhakān vāri-nimagna-dehān 
ān sādhayanty añjana-nasya-lepaiḥ e sādhayanty
añjana-pāna-lepaiḥ
kārpāsāsthi-mayūra-pattra-bṛhatī-nirmālya-piṇḍītaka- ।।

ārpāsāsthi-mayūra-piccha-bṛhatī-nirmālya-piṇḍītaka- -tvaṅ-māṃsī-vṛṣa-daṃśa-viṭ-tuṣa-vacā-keśāhi-nirmokakaiḥ ।।

-tvag-vāṃśī-vṛṣa-daṃśa-viṭ-tuṣa-vacā-keśāhi-nirmocanaiḥ 
-tvag-vāṃśī-vṛṣa-daṃśa-viṇ-nakha-vacā-keśāhi-nirmocanaiḥ
-tvaṅ-māṃsī-vṛṣa-daṃśa-viṭ-tuṣa-vacā-keśāhi-nirmocanaiḥ
nāgendra-dvi-ja-śṛṅga-hiṅgu-maricais tulyaiḥ kṛtaṃ dhūpanaṃ ।।

skandonmāda-piśāca-rākṣasa-surāveśa-jvara-ghnaṃ param ।।
kandonmāda-piśāca-rākṣasa-surāveśa-graha-ghnaṃ param
tri-kaṭuka-dala-kuṅkuma-granthika-kṣāra-siṃhī-niśā-dāru-siddhārtha-yugmāmbu-śakrāhv
ayaiḥ ।।
sita-laśuna-phala-trayośīra-tiktā-vacā-tuttha-yaṣṭī-balā-lohitailā-śilā-padmakaiḥ ।।
dadhi-tagara-madhūka-sāra-priyāhvā-viṣākhyā-viṣā-tārkṣya-śailaiḥ sa-cavyāmayaiḥ kalkitaiḥ ।।

ghṛtam a-navam a-śeṣa-mūtrāṃśa-siddhaṃ mataṃ bhūta-rāvāhvayaṃ pānatas tad graha-ghnaṃ param ।।

nata-madhuka-karañja-lākṣā-paṭolī-samaṅgā-vacā-pāṭalī-hiṅgu-siddhārtha-siṃhī-niśā-yug -latā-rohiṇī- ।।

ata-madhuka-karañja-lākṣā-paṭolī-samaṅgā-vacā-pāṭalā-hiṅgu-siddhārtha-siṃhī-niśā-yug -latā-rohiṇī-

-badara-kaṭu-phala-trikā-kāṇḍa-dāru-kṛmighnājagandhāmarāṅkolla-kośātakī-śigru-nimbā mbu dendrāhvayaiḥ ।।

-badara-kaṭu-phala-trikā-kāṇḍa-dāru-kṛmighnājagandhā-surāṅkolla-kośātakī-śigru-nimbā mbudendrāhvayaiḥ -madana-kaṭu-phala-trikā-kāṇḍa-dāru-kṛmighnājagandhāmarāṅkolla-kośātakī-śigru-nimbā mbudendrāhvayaiḥ adana-kaṭu-phala-trikā-kāṇḍa-dāru-kṛmighnājagandhā-surāṅkolla-kośātakī-śigru-nimbā mbudendrāhvayaiḥ -madana-kaṭu-phala-trikā-kāṇḍa-dāru-kṛmighnājagandhāmṛtā-kola-kośātakī-śigru-nimbā 
mbudendrāhvayaiḥ
gada-śukataru-puṣpa-bījogra-yaṣṭy-adrikarṇī-nikumbhāgni-bilvaiḥ samaiḥ kalkitair
mūtra-vargeṇa siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ ।।

vidhi-vinihitam āśu sarvaiḥ kramair yojitaṃ hanti sarva-grahonmāda-kuṣṭha-jvarāṃs tan mahā-bhūta- rāvaṃ smṛtam ।।

idhi-van nihitam āśu sarvaiḥ kramair yojitaṃ hanti sarva-grahonmāda-kuṣṭha-jvarāṃs tan mahā-bhūta- rāvaṃ smṛtam ira-vinihitam āśu sarvaiḥ kramair yojitaṃ hanti 
sarva-grahonmāda-kuṣṭha-jvarāṃs tan mahā-bhūta-rāvaṃ smṛtam
grahā gṛhṇanti ye yeṣu teṣāṃ teṣu viśeṣataḥ ।
dineṣu bali-homādīn prayuñjīta cikitsakaḥ ।।

snāna-vastra-vasā-māṃsa-madya-kṣīra-guḍādi ca ।
rocate yad yadā yebhyas tat teṣām āharet tadā ।।

nānaṃ vastraṃ vasā māṃsaṃ adyaṃ kṣīra-guḍāni vā
ratnāni gandha-mālyāni bījāni madhu-sarpiṣī ।
bhakṣyāś ca sarve sarveṣāṃ sāmānyo vidhir ity ayam ।।

aktāni gandha-mālyāni hakṣāś ca sarve sarveṣāṃ
surarṣi-guru-vṛddhebhyaḥ siddhebhyaś ca surālaye ।
diśy uttarasyāṃ tatrāpi devāyopahared balim ।।

paścimāyāṃ yathā-kālaṃ daitya-bhūtāya catvare ।
gandharvāya gavāṃ mārge sa-vastrābharaṇaṃ balim ।।

pitṛ-nāga-grahe nadyāṃ nāgebhyaḥ pūrva-dakṣiṇe ।
yakṣāya yakṣāyatane saritor vā samāgame ।।

itṛ-nāma-grahe nadyāṃ
catuṣ-pathe rākṣasāya bhīmeṣu gahaneṣu ca ।
rakṣasāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ tu pūrvasyāṃ brahma-rakṣasām ।।

hīmeṣu gahaneṣu vā
śūnyālaye piśācāya paścimāṃ diśam āsthite ।
śuci-śuklāni mālyāni gandhāḥ kṣaireyam odanam ।।

aścimāṃ diśam āśrite aścimāyāṃ diśi sthite
dadhi cchattraṃ ca dhavalaṃ devānāṃ balir iṣyate ।
hiṅgu-sarṣapa-ṣaḍgranthā-vyoṣair ardha-palonmitaiḥ ।।

catur-guṇe gavāṃ mūtre ghṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।
tat-pāna-nāvanābhyaṅgair deva-graha-vimokṣaṇam ।।

nasyāñjanaṃ vacā-hiṅgu-laśunaṃ basta-vāriṇā ।
daitye balir bahu-phalaḥ sośīra-kamalotpalaḥ ।।

asyāñjane vacā-hiṅgu-
nāgānāṃ sumano-lāja-guḍāpūpa-guḍaudanaiḥ ।
paramānna-madhu-kṣīra-kṛṣṇa-mṛn-nāgakesaraiḥ ।।

vacā-padma-purośīra-raktotpala-dalair baliḥ ।
śvetapattraṃ ca lodhraṃ ca tagaraṃ nāga-sarṣapāḥ ।।

acā-pāṭhā-purośīra-
śītena vāriṇā piṣṭaṃ nāvanāñjanayor hitam ।
yakṣāṇāṃ kṣīra-dadhy-ājya-miśrakaudana-guggulu ।।

devadārūtpalaṃ padmaṃ uśīraṃ vastra-kāñcanam ।
hiraṇyaṃ ca balir yojyo mūtrājya-kṣīram ekataḥ ।।

śīraṃ vastra-candanam śīraṃ vastra-kambalam
siddhaṃ samonmitaṃ pāna-nāvanābhyañjane hitam ।
harītakī haridre dve laśuno maricaṃ vacā ।।

iddhaṃ palonmitaṃ pāna-
nimba-pattraṃ ca bastāmbu-kalkitaṃ nāvanāñjanam ।
brahma-rakṣo-baliḥ siddhaṃ yavānāṃ pūrṇam āḍhakam ।।

avānāṃ cūrṇam āḍhakam
toyasya kumbhaḥ palalaṃ chattraṃ vastram vilepanam ।
gāyatrī-viṃśati-pala-kvāthe ardha-palikaiḥ pacet ।।

oya-kumbhaṃ ca palalaṃ
try-ūṣaṇa-tri-phalā-hiṅgu-ṣaḍgranthā-miśi-sarṣapaiḥ ।
sa-nimba-pattra-laśunaiḥ kuḍavān sapta sarpiṣaḥ ।।

go-mūtre tri-guṇe pāna-nasyābhyaṅgeṣu tad dhitam ।
rakṣasāṃ palalaṃ śuklaṃ kusumaṃ miśrakaudanam ।।

o-mūtre tri-guṇe siddhaṃ ānābhyaṅgeṣu tad dhitam 
kusumaṃ miśrakaudanaḥ
baliḥ pakvāma-māṃsāni niṣpāvā rudhirokṣitāḥ ।
naktamāla-śirīṣa-tvaṅ-mūla-puṣpa-phalāni ca ।।

-mūlaṃ puṣpaṃ phalāni ca -mūle puṣpaṃ phalāni ca
tad-vac ca kṛṣṇa-pāṭalyā bilva-mūlaṃ kaṭu-trikam ।
hiṅgv-indrayava-siddhārtha-laśunāmalakī-phalam ।।

nāvanāñjanayor yojyo basta-mūtra-yuto a-gadaḥ ।
ebhir eva ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ gavāṃ mūtre catur-guṇe ।।

asta-mūtra-hṛto a-gadaḥ asta-mūtra-druto a-gadaḥ
rakṣo-grahān vārayate pānābhyañjana-nāvanaiḥ ।
piśācānāṃ baliḥ sīdhuḥ piṇyākaḥ palalaṃ dadhi ।।

mūlakaṃ lavaṇaṃ sarpiḥ sa-bhūtaudana-yāvakam ।
haridrā-dvaya-mañjiṣṭhā-miśi-saindhava-nāgaram ।।

rabhūtaudana-yāvakam rāg-bhūtaudana-yāvakam 
-miśi-saindhava-nāgaraiḥ
hiṅgu-priyaṅgu-tri-kaṭu-laśuna-tri-phalā vacā ।
pāṭalī-śveta-kaṭabhī-śirīṣa-kusumair ghṛtam ।।

-laśuna-tri-phalā-vacāḥ aṭolī-śveta-kaṭabhī- 
pāṭalā-śveta-kaṭabhī-
go-mūtra-pādikaṃ siddhaṃ pānābhyañjanayor hitam ।
bastāmbu-piṣṭais tair eva yojyam añjana-nāvanam ।।

devarṣi-pitṛ-gandharve tīkṣṇaṃ nasyādi varjayet ।
sarpiḥ-pānādi mṛasmin bhaiṣajyam avacārayet ।।

ṛte piśācāt sarveṣu pratikūlaṃ ca nācaret ।
sa-vaidyam āturaṃ ghnanti kruddhās te hi mahaujasaḥ ।।

īśvaraṃ dvā-daśa-bhujaṃ nātham āryāvalokitam ।
sarva-vyādhi-cikitsāṃ ca japan sarva-grahān jayet ।।

arva-vyādhi-cikitsantaṃ arva-vyādhi-cikitsaṃ ca 
sarva-vyādhi-cikitsitaṃ
tathonmādān apasmārān anyaṃ vā citta-viplavam ।
mahā-vidyāṃ ca māyūrīṃ śuciṃ taṃ śrāvayet sadā ।।

nyān vā citta-vibhramān śucis taṃ śrāvayet sadā
bhūteśaṃ pūjayet sthāṇuṃ pramathākhyāṃś ca tad-gaṇān ।
japan siddhāṃś ca tan-mantrān grahān sarvān apohati ।।

yac cān-antarayoḥ kiñ-cid vakṣyate adhyāyayor hitam ।
yac coktam iha tat sarvaṃ prayuñjīta paras-param ।।

athoktam iha tat sarvaṃ

uttarasthāna
unmādāḥ ṣaṭ pṛthag-doṣa-nicayādhi-viṣodbhavāḥ ।
unmādo nāma manaso doṣair unmārga-gair madaḥ ।।

śārīra-mānasair duṣṭair a-hitād anna-pānataḥ ।
vikṛtā-sātmya-sa-malād viṣamād upayogataḥ ।।

śārīra-mānasair doṣair ikṛtā-sātmya-sa-mala- -viṣamād 
upayogataḥ
viṣaṇṇasyālpa-sat-tvasya vyādhi-vega-samudgamāt ।
kṣīṇasya ceṣṭā-vaiṣamyāt pūjya-pūjā-vyatikramāt ।।

yādhi-vega-samudbhavāt yādhi-vega-samudbhramāt
ādhibhir citta-vibhraṃśād viṣeṇopaviṣeṇa ca ।
ebhir hi hīna-sat-tvasya hṛdi doṣāḥ pradūṣitāḥ ।।

iṣeṇopaviṣeṇa vā bhir vihīna-sat-tvasya
dhiyo vidhāya kāluṣyaṃ hṛtvā mārgān mano-vahān ।
unmādaṃ kurvate tena dhī-vijñāna-smṛti-bhramāt ।।

deho duḥkha-sukha-bhraṣṭo bhraṣṭa-sārathi-vad rathaḥ ।
bhramaty a-cintitārambhas tatra vātāt kṛśāṅga-tā ।।

ehī duḥkha-sukha-bhraṣṭo
a-sthāne rodanākrośa-hasita-smita-nartanam ।
gīta-vāditra-vāg-aṅga-vikṣepāsphoṭanāni ca ।।

a-sāmnā veṇu-vīṇādi-śabdānukaraṇaṃ muhuḥ ।
āsyāt phenāgamo ajasram aṭanaṃ bahu-bhāṣi-tā ।।

bhīkṣṇaṃ veṇu-vīṇādi- āsyena veṇu-vīṇādi- -śabdādi-karaṇaṃ muhuḥ 
ṭanaṃ bahu-bhāṣitam
alaṅkāro an-alaṅkārair a-yānair gamanodyamaḥ ।
gṛddhir abhyavahāryeṣu tal-lābhe cāvamāna-tā ।।

al-lābhe vāvamāna-tā al-lābheṣv avamāna-tā
utpiṇḍitāruṇākṣi-tvaṃ jīrṇe cānne gadodbhavaḥ ।
pittāt saṃtarjanaṃ krodho muṣṭi-loṣṭādy-abhidravaḥ ।।

tpīḍitāruṇākṣi-tvaṃ
śīta-cchāyodakākāṅkṣā nagna-tvaṃ pīta-varṇa-tā ।
a-satya-jvalana-jvālā-tārakā-dīpa-darśanam ।।

etra-tvak-pīta-varṇa-tā -sati jvalane jvālā- 
a-satya-jvalanolkādi-
kaphād a-rocakaś chardir alpehāhāra-vākya-tā ।
strī-kāma-tā rahaḥ-prītir lālā-siṅghāṇaka-srutiḥ ।।

baibhatsyaṃ śauca-vidveṣo nidrā śvayathur ānane ।
unmādo bala-vān rātrau bhukta-mātre ca jāyate ।।

sarvāyatana-saṃsthāna-saṃnipāte tad-ātmakam ।
unmādaṃ dāruṇaṃ vidyāt taṃ bhiṣak parivarjayet ।।

-saṃnipātāt tad-ātmakam
dhana-kāntādi-nāśena duḥ-sahenābhiṣaṅga-vān ।
pāṇḍur dīno muhur muhyan hāheti paridevate ।।

rodity a-kasmān mriyate tad-guṇān bahu manyate ।
śoka-kliṣṭa-manā dhyāyañ jāgarūko viceṣṭate ।।

odity a-kasmāt smayate
viṣeṇa śyāva-vadano naṣṭa-cchāyā-balendriyaḥ ।
vegāntare api saṃbhrānto raktākṣas taṃ vivarjayet ।।

aṣṭa-cchāyo a-balendriyaḥ
athānila-ja unmāde sneha-pānaṃ prayojayet ।
pūrvam āvṛta-mārge tu sa-snehaṃ mṛdu śodhanam ।।

kapha-pitta-bhave apy ādau vamanaṃ sa-virecanam ।
snigdha-svinnasya vastiṃ ca śirasaḥ sa-virecanam ।।

apha-pittodbhave apy ādau nigdha-svinnasya vastīṃś ca 
śirasaś ca virecanam
tathāsya śuddha-dehasya prasādaṃ labhate manaḥ ।
ittham apy anuvṛttau tu tīkṣṇaṃ nāvanam añjanam ।।

athaiva śuddha-dehasya
harṣaṇāśvāsanottrāsa-bhaya-tāḍana-tarjanam ।
abhyaṅgodvartanālepa-dhūpān pānaṃ ca sarpiṣaḥ ।।

-dhūmān pānaṃ ca sarpiṣaḥ
yuñjyāt tāni hi śuddhasya nayanti prakṛtiṃ manaḥ ।
hiṅgu-sauvarcala-vyoṣair dvi-palāṃśair ghṛtāḍhakam ।।

siddhaṃ sa-mūtram unmāda-bhūtāpasmāra-nut param ।
dvau prasthau sva-rasād brāhmyā ghṛta-prasthaṃ ca sādhitam ।।

vyoṣa-śyāmā-trivṛd-dantī-śaṅkhapuṣpī-nṛpadrumaiḥ ।
sa-saptalā-kṛmiharaiḥ kalkitair akṣa-saṃmitaiḥ ।।

yoṣa-śyāmā-trivṛd-bimbī- ātalā-kṛmijit-kalkaiḥ arvais 
tair akṣa-saṃmitaiḥ
pala-vṛddhyā prayuñjīta paraṃ mātrā catuḥ-palam ।
unmāda-kuṣṭhāpasmāra-haraṃ vandhyā-suta-pradam ।।

vāk-svara-smṛti-medhā-kṛd dhanyaṃ brāhmī-ghṛtaṃ smṛtam ।
varā-viśālā-bhadrailā-devadārv-elavālukaiḥ ।।

arā-viśālākautpalā- arā-viśālā-pattrailā-
dvi-śārivā-dvi-rajanī-dvi-sthirā-phalinī-nataiḥ ।
bṛhatī-kuṣṭha-mañjiṣṭhā-nāgakesara-dāḍimaiḥ ।।

vella-tālīśa-pattrailā-mālatī-mukulotpalaiḥ ।
sa-dantī-padmaka-himaiḥ karṣāṃśaiḥ sarpiṣaḥ pacet ।।

-mālatī-kumudotpalaiḥ udantī-padmaka-himaiḥ
prasthaṃ bhūta-grahonmāda-kāsāpasmāra-pāpmasu ।
pāṇḍu-kaṇḍū-viṣe śoṣe mohe mehe gare jvare ।।

-kāsāpasmāra-pāpma-jit āṇḍu-kaṇḍū-viṣe śophe
a-retasy a-prajasi vā daivopahata-cetasi ।
a-medhasi skhalad-vāci smṛti-kāme alpa-pāvake ।।

-retasy alpa-rajasi
balyaṃ maṅgalyam āyuṣyaṃ kānti-saubhāgya-puṣṭi-dam ।
kalyāṇakam idaṃ sarpiḥ śreṣṭhaṃ puṃ-savaneṣu ca ।।

ebhyo dvi-śārivādīni jale paktvaika-viṃśatim ।
rase tasmin pacet sarpir gṛṣṭi-kṣīra-catur-guṇam ।।

ṛṣṭi-kṣīre catur-guṇe ṛṣṭi-kṣīraṃ catur-guṇam
vīrā-dvi-medā-kākolī-kapikacchū-viṣāṇibhiḥ ।
śūrpaparṇī-yutair etan mahā-kalyāṇakaṃ param ।।

īrarddhi-medā-kākolī- ahā-kalyāṇakaṃ smṛtam
bṛṃhaṇaṃ saṃnipāta-ghnaṃ pūrvasmād adhikaṃ guṇaiḥ ।
jaṭilā pūtanā keśī cāraṭī markaṭī vacā ।।

trāyamāṇā jayā vīrā corakaḥ kaṭu-rohiṇī ।
vayaḥsthā śūkarī chattrā sāticchattrā palaṅkaṣā ।।

ticchattrā palaṅkaṣā
mahāpuruṣadantā ca kāyasthā nākulī-dvayam ।
kaṭambharā vṛścikālī śāliparṇī ca tair ghṛtam ।।

aṭambharā-vṛścikālī- -sthirāś cāhṛtya tair ghṛtam
siddhaṃ cāturthikonmāda-grahāpasmāra-nāśanam ।
mahā-paiśācakaṃ nāma ghṛtam etad yathāmṛtam ।।

iddhaṃ caturthakonmāda- iddhaṃ cāturthakonmāda-
buddhi-medhā-smṛti-karaṃ bālānāṃ cāṅga-vardhanam ।
brāhmīm aindrīṃ viḍaṅgāni vyoṣaṃ hiṅgu jaṭāṃ murām ।।

mṛti-buddhi-karaṃ caiva ālānām aṅga-vardhanam
rāsnāṃ viṣaghnāṃ laśunaṃ viśalyāṃ surasāṃ vacām ।
jyotiṣmatīṃ nāgavinnām anantāṃ sa-harītakīm ।।

āsnāṃ viṣaghnīṃ laśunaṃ
kāṅkṣīṃ ca hasti-mūtreṇa piṣṭvā chāyā-viśoṣītā ।
vartir nasyāñjanālepa-dhūpair unmāda-sūdanī ।।

ācchīṃ ca hasti-mūtreṇa aurāṣṭrīṃ basta-mūtreṇa 
-dhūpair unmāda-nāśinī
avapīḍāś ca vividhāḥ sarṣapāḥ sneha-saṃyutāḥ ।
kaṭu-tailena cābhyaṅgo dhmāpayec cāsya tad rajaḥ ।।

sa-hiṅgus tīkṣṇa-dhūmaś ca sūtra-sthānodito hitaḥ ।
śṛgāla-śalyakolūka-jalaukā-vṛṣa-basta-jaiḥ ।।

a-hiṅgu tīkṣṇa-dhūmaś ca -jalūkā-vṛṣa-basta-jaiḥ 
-jalaukā-vṛka-basta-jaiḥ
mūtra-pitta-śakṛd-roma-nakha-carmabhir ācaret ।
dhūpa-dhūmāñjanābhyaṅga-pradeha-pariṣecanam ।।

dhūpayet satataṃ cainaṃ śva-go-matsyaiḥ su-pūtibhiḥ ।
vāta-śleṣmātmake prāyaḥ paittike tu praśasyate ।।

tiktakaṃ jīvanīyaṃ ca sarpiḥ snehaś ca miśrakaḥ ।
śītāni cānna-pānāni madhurāṇi laghūni ca ।।

vidhyet sirāṃ yathoktāṃ vā tṛptaṃ medyāmiṣasya vā ।
nivāte śāyayed evaṃ mucyate mati-vibhramāt ।।

idhyet sirāṃ yathoktāṃ ca
prakṣipyā-salile kūpe śoṣayed vā bubhukṣayā ।
āśvāsayet suhṛt taṃ vā vākyair dharmārtha-saṃhitaiḥ ।।

āśvāsayet suhṛdbhis taṃ
brūyād iṣṭa-vināśaṃ vā darśayed adbhutāni vā ।
baddhaṃ sarṣapa-tailāktaṃ nyased vottānam ātape ।।

rūyād iṣṭasya nāśaṃ vā yastaṃ cottānam ātape
kapikacchvātha-vā taptair loha-taila-jalaiḥ spṛśet ।
kaśābhis tāḍayitvā vā baddhaṃ śvabhre viniḥkṣipet ।।

addhvā śvabhre viniḥkṣipet
atha-vā vīta-śastrāśma-jane saṃtamase gṛhe ।
sarpeṇoddhṛta-daṃṣṭreṇa dāntaiḥ siṃhair gajaiś ca tam ।।
trāsayec chastra-hastair vā kirātārāti-taskaraiḥ ।।
taskaraiḥ śatrubhis tathā
atha-vā rāja-puruṣā bahir nītvā su-saṃyatam ।
bhāpayeyur vadhenainaṃ tarjayanto nṛpājñayā ।।

deha-duḥkha-bhayebhyo hi paraṃ prāṇa-bhayaṃ matam ।
tena yāti śamaṃ tasya sarvato viplutaṃ manaḥ ।।

arvato apasṛtaṃ manaḥ
siddhā kriyā prayojyeyaṃ deśa-kālādy-apekṣayā ।
iṣṭa-dravya-vināśāt tu mano yasyopahanyate ।।

iddhāḥ kriyā prayoktavyā
tasya tat-sadṛśa-prāpti-sāntvāśvāsaiḥ śamaṃ nayet ।
kāma-śoka-bhaya-krodha-harṣerṣyā-lobha-saṃbhavān ।।

asya tat-sadṛśa-prāptiḥ -sāntvāśvāsaiḥ prasādayet -priyāśvāsaiḥ pradarśayet 
āntvāśvāsaiḥ śamaṃ nayet
paras-para-prati-dvandvair ebhir eva śamaṃ nayet ।
bhūtānubandham īkṣeta prokta-liṅgādhikākṛtim ।।

hūtānubaddham īkṣeta
yady unmāde tataḥ kuryād bhūta-nirdiṣṭam auṣadham ।
baliṃ ca dadyāt palalaṃ yāvakaṃ saktu-piṇḍikām ।।

ady unmāde ca tat kuryād
snigdhaṃ madhuram āhāraṃ taṇḍulān rudhirokṣitān ।
pakvāmakāni māṃsāni surāṃ maireyam āsavam ।।

akvāmāhvāni māṃsāni urā-maireyam āsavam
atimuktasya puṣpāṇi jātyāḥ sahacarasya ca ।
catuṣ-pathe gavāṃ tīrthe nadīnāṃ saṃgameṣu ca ।।

nivṛttāmiṣa-madyo yo hitāśī prayataḥ śuciḥ ।
nijāgantubhir unmādaiḥ sat-tva-vān na sa yujyate ।।

ivṛttāmiṣa-madyo api
prasāda indriyārthānāṃ buddhy-ātma-manasāṃ tathā ।
dhātūnāṃ prakṛti-stha-tvaṃ vigatonmāda-lakṣaṇam ।।

ndriyāṇāṃ prasanna-tvaṃ atonmādasya lakṣaṇam

uttarasthāna
smṛty-apāyo hy apasmāraḥ sa dhī-sat-tvābhisaṃplavāt ।
jāyate abhihate citte cintā-śoka-bhayādibhiḥ ।।

a dhī-sat-tvādi-saṃplavāt
unmāda-vat prakupitaiś citta-deha-gatair malaiḥ ।
hate sat-tve hṛdi vyāpte saṃjñā-vāhiṣu kheṣu ca ।।

tamo viśan mūḍha-matir bībhatsāḥ kurute kriyāḥ ।
dantān khādan vaman phenaṃ hastau pādau ca vikṣipan ।।

astau pādau ca kampayan
paśyann a-santi rūpāṇi praskhalan patati kṣitau ।
vijihmākṣi-bhruvo doṣa-vege atīte vibudhyate ।।

kālāntareṇa sa punaś caivam eva viceṣṭate ।
apasmāraś catur-bhedo vātādyair nicayena ca ।।

rūpam utpatsyamāne asmin hṛt-kampaḥ śūnya-tā bhramaḥ ।
tamaso darśanaṃ dhyānaṃ bhrū-vyudāso akṣi-vaikṛtam ।।

ūpam utpadyamāne asmin
a-śabda-śravaṇaṃ svedo lālā-siṅghāṇaka-srutiḥ ।
a-vipāko a-rucir mūrchā kukṣy-āṭopo bala-kṣayaḥ ।।

nidrā-nāśo aṅga-mardas tṛṭ svapne gānaṃ sa-nartanam ।
pānaṃ tailasya madyasya tayor eva ca mehanam ।।

tatra vātāt sphurat-sakthiḥ prapataṃś ca muhur muhuḥ ।
apasmarati saṃjñāṃ ca labhate vi-svaraṃ rudan ।।

ratataṃ ca muhur muhuḥ
utpiṇḍitākṣaḥ śvasiti phenaṃ vamati kampate ।
āvidhyati śiro dantān daśaty ādhmāta-kandharaḥ ।।

parito vikṣipaty aṅgaṃ viṣamaṃ vinatāṅguliḥ ।
rūkṣa-śyāvāruṇākṣi-tvaṅ-nakhāsyaḥ kṛṣṇam īkṣate ।।

capalaṃ paruṣaṃ rūpaṃ vi-rūpaṃ vikṛtānanam ।
apasmarati pittena muhuḥ saṃjñāṃ ca vindati ।।

apalaṃ paramaṃ rūpaṃ apalaṃ paruṣaṃ rūkṣaṃ
pīta-phenākṣi-vaktra-tvag āsphālayati medinīm ।
bhairavādīpta-ruṣita-rūpa-darśī tṛṣānvitaḥ ।।

kaphāc cireṇa grahaṇaṃ cireṇaiva vibodhanam ।
ceṣṭālpā bhūyasī lālā śukla-netra-nakhāsya-tā ।।

śuklābha-rūpa-darśi-tvaṃ sarva-liṅgaṃ tu varjayet ।
athāvṛtānāṃ dhī-citta-hṛt-khānāṃ prāk-prabodhanam ।।

tīkṣṇaiḥ kuryād apasmāre karmabhir vamanādibhiḥ ।
vātikaṃ vasti-bhūyiṣṭhaiḥ paittaṃ prāyo virecanaiḥ ।।

ślaiṣmikaṃ vamana-prāyair apasmāram upācaret ।
sarvataḥ su-viśuddhasya samyag āśvāsitasya ca ।।

apasmāra-vimokṣārthaṃ yogān saṃśamanāñ chṛṇu ।
go-maya-sva-rasa-kṣīra-dadhi-mūtraiḥ śṛtaṃ haviḥ ।।

apasmāra-jvaronmāda-kāmalānta-karaṃ pibet ।
dvi-pañca-mūla-tri-phalā-dvi-niśā-kuṭaja-tvacaḥ ।।

vi-pañca-mūlī-tri-phalā-
saptaparṇam apāmārgaṃ nīlinīṃ kaṭu-rohiṇīm ।
śamyāka-puṣkara-jaṭā-phalgu-mūla-durālabhāḥ ।।

śyoṇāka-puṣkara-jaṭā-
dvi-palāḥ salila-droṇe paktvā pādāvaśeṣite ।
bhārgī-pāṭhāḍhakī-kumbha-nikumbha-vyoṣa-rohiṣaiḥ ।।

vi-palāni jala-droṇe
mūrvā-bhūtika-bhūnimba-śreyasī-śārivā-dvayaiḥ ।
madayanty-agni-niculair akṣāṃśaiḥ sarpiṣaḥ pacet ।।

ūrvā-pūtika-bhūnimba-
prasthaṃ tad-vad dravaiḥ pūrvaiḥ pañca-gavyam idaṃ mahat ।
jvarāpasmāra-jaṭhara-bhagandara-haraṃ param ।।

śophārśaḥ-kāmalā-pāṇḍu-gulma-kāsa-grahāpaham ।
brāhmī-rasa-vacā-kuṣṭha-śaṅkhapuṣpī-śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।।

-gulma-kāsa-bhramāpaham
purāṇaṃ medhyam unmādā-lakṣmy-apasmāra-pāpma-jit ।
taila-prasthaṃ ghṛta-prasthaṃ jīvanīyaiḥ palonmitaiḥ ।।

kṣīra-droṇe pacet siddham apasmāra-vimokṣaṇam ।
kaṃse kṣīrekṣu-rasayoḥ kāśmarye aṣṭa-guṇe rase ।।

kārṣikair jīvanīyaiś ca sarpiḥ-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।
vāta-pittodbhavaṃ kṣipram apasmāraṃ nihanti tat ।।

tad-vat kāśa-vidārīkṣu-kuśa-kvātha-śṛtaṃ payaḥ ।
kūṣmāṇḍa-sva-rase sarpir aṣṭā-daśa-guṇe śṛtam ।।

-kuśa-kvāthe śṛtaṃ payaḥ -kuśa-kvāthaiḥ śṛtaṃ payaḥ
yaṣṭī-kalkam apasmāra-haraṃ dhī-vāk-svara-pradam ।
kapilānāṃ gavāṃ pittaṃ nāvane paramaṃ hitam ।।

aṣṭī-kalkaṃ apasmāraṃ āvanaṃ paramaṃ hitam 
hared dhī-vāk-svara-pradam
śva-śṛgāla-biḍālānāṃ siṃhādīnāṃ ca pūjitam ।
godhā-nakula-nāgānāṃ pṛṣatarkṣa-gavām api ।।

ṛṣabharkṣa-gavām api ṛka-carka-gavām api
pitteṣu sādhitaṃ tailaṃ nasye abhyaṅge ca śasyate ।
tri-phalā-vyoṣa-pītadru-yava-kṣāra-phaṇijjakaiḥ ।।

itteṣu sādhayet tailaṃ asyābhyaṅgeṣu śasyate
śry-āhvāpāmārga-kārañja-bījais tailaṃ vipācitam ।
basta-mūtre hitaṃ nasyaṃ cūrṇaṃ vā dhmāpayed bhiṣak ।।

śyāmāpāmārga-kārañja- -bījais tailaṃ prasādhitam 
-bījais tailaṃ vipācayet
nakulolūka-mārjāra-gṛdhra-kīṭāhi-kāka-jaiḥ ।
tuṇḍaiḥ pakṣaiḥ purīṣaiś ca dhūpam asya prayojayet ।।

hūmam asya prayojayet hūpam asmai prayojayet
śīlayet taila-laśunaṃ payasā vā śatāvarīm ।
brāhmī-rasaṃ kuṣṭha-rasaṃ vacāṃ vā madhu-saṃyutām ।।

samaṃ kruddhair apasmāro doṣaiḥ śārīra-mānasaiḥ ।
yaj jāyate yataś caiṣa mahā-marma-samāśrayaḥ ।।

tasmād rasāyanair enaṃ duś-cikitsyam upācaret ।
tad-ārtaṃ cāgni-toyāder viṣamāt pālayet sadā ।।

asmād rasāyanenainaṃ ad-ārtaṃ cāgni-toyādi- -viṣamāt 
pālayet sadā
muktaṃ mano-vikāreṇa tvam itthaṃ kṛta-vān iti ।
na brūyād viṣayair iṣṭaiḥ kliṣṭaṃ ceto asya bṛṃhayet ।।

uttarasthāna
sarva-roga-nidānoktair a-hitaiḥ kupitā malāḥ ।
a-cakṣuṣyair viśeṣeṇa prāyaḥ pittānusāriṇaḥ ।।

sirābhir ūrdhvaṃ prasṛtā netrāvayavam āśritāḥ ।
vartma saṃdhiṃ sitaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dṛṣṭiṃ vā sarvam akṣi vā ।।

rogān kuryuś calas tatra prāpya vartmāśrayāḥ sirāḥ ।
suptotthitasya kurute vartma-stambhaṃ sa-vedanam ।।

pāṃsu-pūrṇābha-netra-tvaṃ kṛcchronmīlanam aśru ca ।
vimardanāt syāc ca śamaḥ kṛcchronmūlaṃ vadanti tat ।।

cālayan vartmanī vāyur nimeṣonmeṣaṇaṃ muhuḥ ।
karoty a-ruṅ nimeṣo asau vartma yat tu nimīlyate ।।

vimukta-saṃdhi niś-ceṣṭaṃ hīnaṃ vāta-hataṃ hi tat ।
kṛṣṇāḥ pittena bahvyo antar-vartma kumbhīka-bīja-vat ।।

ittena vartmano antar-jā ahvyaḥ kumbhīka-bīja-vat
ādhmāyante punar bhinnāḥ piṭikāḥ kumbhi-saṃjñitāḥ ।
sa-dāha-kleda-nistodaṃ raktābhaṃ sparśanā-kṣamam ।।

iṭikāḥ kumbhi-saṃjñakāḥ
pittena jāyate vartma pittotkliṣṭam uśanti tat ।
karoti kaṇḍūṃ dāhaṃ ca pittaṃ pakṣṃāntam āsthitam ।।

ittaṃ pakṣṃāntam āśritam
pakṣmaṇāṃ śātanaṃ cānu pakṣma-śātaṃ vadanti tam ।
pothakyaḥ piṭikāḥ śvetāḥ sarṣapābhā ghanāḥ kaphāt ।।

akṣmaṇāṃ śatanaṃ cānu akṣmaṇāṃ sadanaṃ cānu
śophopadeha-ruk-kaṇḍū-picchilāśru-samanvitāḥ ।
kaphotkliṣṭaṃ bhaved vartma stambha-kledopadeha-vat ।।

granthiḥ pāṇḍura-ruk-pākaḥ kaṇḍū-mān kaṭhinaḥ kaphāt ।
kola-mātraḥ sa lagaṇaḥ kiñ-cid alpas tato atha-vā ।।

iñ-cid alpas tato api vā
raktā raktena piṭikā tat-tulya-piṭikācitā ।
utsaṅgākhyā tathotkliṣṭaṃ rājī-mat sparśanā-kṣamam ।।

aktā raktena piṭikās at-tulya-piṭikācitāḥ tsaṅgākhyās 
tathotkliṣṭaṃ
arśo adhi-māṃsaṃ vartmāntaḥ stabdhaṃ snigdhaṃ sa-dāha-ruk ।
raktaṃ raktena tat-srāvi cchinnaṃ chinnaṃ ca vardhate ।।

madhye vā vartmano ante vā kaṇḍūṣā-rug-vatī sthirā ।
mudga-mātrāsṛjā tāmrā piṭikāñjana-nāmikā ।।

doṣair vartma bahiḥ śūnaṃ yad antaḥ sūkṣma-khācitam ।
sa-srāvam antar-udakaṃ bisābhaṃ bisa-vartma tat ।।

yad vartmotkliṣṭam utkliṣṭam a-kasmān mlāna-tām iyāt ।
rakta-doṣa-trayotkleśād bhavaty utkliṣṭa-vartma tat ।।

adanty utkliṣṭa-vartma tat
śyāva-vartma malaiḥ sāsraiḥ śyāvaṃ ruk-kleda-śopha-vat ।
śliṣṭākhyaṃ vartmanī śliṣṭe kaṇḍū-śvayathu-rāgiṇī ।।

vartmano antaḥ kharā rūkṣāḥ piṭikāḥ sikatopamāḥ ।
sikatā-vartma kṛṣṇaṃ tu kardamaṃ kardamopamam ।।

bahalaṃ bahalair māṃsaiḥ sa-varṇaiś cīyate samaiḥ ।
kukūṇakaḥ śiśor eva dantotpatti-nimitta-jaḥ ।।

syāt tena śiśur ucchūna-tāmrākṣo vīkṣaṇā-kṣamaḥ ।
sa-vartma-śūla-paicchilyaḥ karṇa-nāsākṣi-mardanaḥ ।।

-tāmrākṣo vīkṣaṇe a-kṣamaḥ
pakṣmoparodhe saṃkoco vartmanāṃ jāyate tathā ।
khara-tāntar-mukha-tvaṃ ca romṇām anyāni vā punaḥ ।।

artmano jāyate tathā
kaṇṭakair iva tīkṣṇāgrair ghṛṣṭaṃ tair akṣi śūyate ।
uṣyate cānilādi-dviḍ alpāhaḥ śāntir uddhṛtaiḥ ।।

hṛṣṭaṃ tair akṣi sūyate ṣyate vānilādi-dviḍ ṣyate cānilādyaiś ca 
lpāhaṃ śāntir uddhṛtaiḥ
kanīnake bahir-vartma kaṭhino granthir unnataḥ ।
tāmraḥ pakvo asra-pūya-srud alajy ādhmāyate muhuḥ ।।

vartmāntar māṃsa-piṇḍābhaḥ śvayathur grathito a-rujaḥ ।
sāsraiḥ syād arbudo doṣair viṣamo bāhyataś calaḥ ।।

catur-viṃśatir ity ete vyādhayo vartma-saṃśrayāḥ ।
ādyo atra bheṣajaiḥ sādhyo dvau tato arśaś ca varyajet ।।

pakṣmoparodho yāpyaḥ syāc cheṣāñ chastreṇa sādhayet ।
kuṭṭayet pakṣma-sadanaṃ chindyāt teṣv api cārbudam ।।

uṭṭayet pakṣma-śadanaṃ
bhindyāl lagaṇa-kumbhīkā-bisotsaṅgāñjanālajīḥ ।
pothakī-śyāva-sikatā-śliṣṭotkliṣṭa-catuṣṭayam ।।
sa-kardamaṃ sa-bahalaṃ vilikhet sa-kukūṇakam ।।
uttarasthāna
kṛcchronmīle purāṇājyaṃ drākṣā-kalkāmbu-sādhitam ।
sa-sitaṃ yojayet snigdhaṃ nasya-dhūmāñjanādi ca ।।

kumbhīkā-vartma-likhitaṃ saindhava-pratisāritam ।
yaṣṭī-dhātrī-paṭolīnāṃ kvāthena pariṣecayet ।।

nivāte adhiṣṭhitasyāptaiḥ śuddhasyottāna-śāyinaḥ ।
bahiḥ koṣṇāmbu-taptena sveditaṃ vartma vāsasā ।।

nirbhujya vastrāntaritaṃ vāmāṅguṣṭhāṅgulī-ghṛtam ।
na sraṃsate calati vā vartmaivaṃ sarvatas tataḥ ।।

a sraṃsate na calati
maṇḍalāgreṇa tat tiryak kṛtvā śastra-padāṅkitam ।
likhet tenaiva pattrair vā śāka-śephālikādi-jaiḥ ।।

śāka-śephālikādikaiḥ śāka-śephālikādibhiḥ
phenena toya-rāśer vā picunā pramṛjann asṛk ।
sthite rakte su-likhitaṃ sa-kṣaudraiḥ pratisārayet ।।

yathā-svam uktair anu ca prakṣālyoṣṇena vāriṇā ।
ghṛtena siktam abhyaktaṃ badhnīyān madhu-sarpiṣā ।।

hṛtenāsiktam abhyaktaṃ
ūrdhvādhaḥ karṇayor dattvā piṇḍīṃ ca yava-saktubhiḥ ।
dvitīye ahani muktasya pariṣekaṃ yathā-yatham ।।

kuryāc caturthe nasyādīn muñced evāhni pañcame ।
samaṃ nakha-nibhaṃ śopha-kaṇḍū-gharṣādya-pīḍitam ।।

vidyāt su-likhitaṃ vartma likhed bhūyo viparyaye ।
ruk-pakṣma-vartma-sadana-sraṃsanāny ati-lekhanāt ।।

sneha-svedādikas tasminn iṣṭo vāta-haraḥ kramaḥ ।
abhyajya nava-nītena śveta-lodhraṃ pralepayet ।।

eraṇḍa-mūla-kalkena puṭa-pāke pacet tataḥ ।
svinnaṃ prakṣālitaṃ śuṣkaṃ cūrṇitaṃ poṭalī-kṛtam ।।

striyāḥ kṣīre chagalyā vā mṛditaṃ netra-secanam ।
śāli-taṇḍula-kalkena liptaṃ tad-vat pariṣkṛtam ।।

triyāḥ kṣīre chāgale vā
kuryān netre ati-likhite mṛditaṃ dadhi-mastunā ।
kevalenāpi vā sekaṃ mastunā jāṅgalāśinaḥ ।।

piṭikā vrīhi-vaktreṇa bhittvā tu kaṭhinonnatāḥ ।
niṣpīḍayed anu vidhiḥ pariśeṣas tu pūrva-vat ।।

iṭikāṃ vrīhi-vaktreṇa hittvā tu kaṭhinonnatām
lekhane bhedane cāyaṃ kramaḥ sarva-tra vartmani ।
pittāsrotkliṣṭayoḥ svādu-skandha-siddhena sarpiṣā ।।

sirā-vimokṣaḥ snigdhasya trivṛc chreṣṭhaṃ virecanam ।
likhite sruta-rakte ca vartmani kṣālanaṃ hitam ।।

rivṛc chreṣṭhā virecane ikhite niḥsṛte rakte
yaṣṭī-kaṣāyaḥ sekas tu kṣīraṃ candana-sādhitam ।
pakṣmaṇāṃ sadane sūcyā roma-kūpān vikuṭṭayet ।।

aṣṭī-kvāthena sekas tu
grāhayed vā jalaukobhiḥ payasekṣu-rasena vā ।
vamanaṃ nāvanaṃ sarpiḥ śṛtaṃ madhura-śītalaiḥ ।।

saṃcūrṇya puṣpa-kāsīsaṃ bhāvayet surasā-rasaiḥ ।
tāmre daśāhaṃ paramaṃ pakṣma-śāte tad añjanam ।।

pothakīr likhitāḥ śuṇṭhī-saindhava-pratisāritāḥ ।
uṣṇāmbu-kṣālitāḥ siñcet khadirāḍhaki-śigrubhiḥ ।।

othakīṃ likhitaṃ śuṇṭhī- -saindhava-pratisāritām 
uṣṇāmbu-kṣālitāṃ siñcet
ap-siddhair dvi-niṣā-śreṣṭhā-madhukair vā sa-mākṣikaiḥ ।
kaphotkliṣṭe vilikhite sa-kṣaudraiḥ pratisāraṇam ।।

sūkṣmaiḥ saindhava-kāsīsa-manohvā-kaṇa-tārkṣya-jaiḥ ।
vamanāñjana-nasyādi sarvaṃ ca kapha-jid dhitam ।।

kartavyaṃ lagaṇe apy etad a-śāntāv agninā dahet ।
kukūṇe khadira-śreṣṭhā-nimba-pattra-śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।।

-nimba-pattraiḥ śṛtaṃ ghṛtam
svinnāṃ bhittvā viniṣpīḍya bhiṣag añjana-nāmikām ।
śilailā-saindhava-nataiḥ sa-kṣaudraiḥ pratisārayet ।।

svinnāṃ bhittvā viniṣpīḍyotṃ ṃsaṅgāṃ 
cāñjana-nāmikām
pītvā dhātrī vamet kṛṣṇā-yaṣṭī-sarṣapa-saindhavaiḥ ।
abhayā-pippalī-drākṣā-kvāthenaināṃ virecayet ।।

mustā-dvi-rajanī-kṛṣṇā-kalkenālepayet stanau ।
dhūpayet sarṣapaiḥ sājyaiḥ śuddhāṃ kvāthaṃ ca pāyayet ।।

paṭola-musta-mṛdvīkā-guḍūcī-tri-phalodbhavam ।
śiśos tu likhitaṃ vartma srutāsṛg vāmbu-janmabhiḥ ।।

dhātry-aśmantaka-jambūttha-pattra-kvāthena secayet ।
prāyaḥ kṣīra-ghṛtāśi-tvād bālānāṃ śleṣma-jā gadāḥ ।।

tasmād vamanam evāgre sarva-vyādhiṣu pūjitam ।
sindhūttha-kṛṣṇāpāmārga-bījājya-stanya-mākṣikam ।।

cūrṇo vacāyāḥ sa-kṣaudro madanaṃ madhukānvitam ।
kṣīraṃ kṣīrānnam annaṃ ca bhajataḥ kramataḥ śiśoḥ ।।

hajataḥ krama-śaḥ śiśoḥ
vamanaṃ sarva-rogeṣu viśeṣeṇa kukūṇake ।
saptalā-rasa-siddhājyaṃ yojyaṃ cobhaya-śodhanam ।।

dvi-niśā-lodhra-yaṣṭy-āhva-rohiṇī-nimba-pallavaiḥ ।
kukūṇake hitā vartiḥ piṣṭais tāmra-rajo-'nvitaiḥ ।।

kṣīra-kṣaudra-ghṛtopetaṃ dagdhaṃ vā loha-jaṃ rajaḥ ।
elā-laśuna-kataka-śaṅkhoṣaṇa-phaṇijjakaiḥ ।।

agdhaṃ vā lodhra-jaṃ rajaḥ
vartiḥ kukūṇa-pothakyoḥ surā-piṣṭaiḥ sa-kaṭphalaiḥ ।
pakṣma-rodhe pravṛddheṣu śuddha-dehasya romasu ।।

utsṛjya dvau bhruvo adhas-tād bhāgau bhāgaṃ ca pakṣmataḥ ।
yava-mātraṃ yavākāraṃ tiryak chittvārdra-vāsasā ।।

apaneyam asṛk tasminn alpī-bhavati śoṇite ।
sīvyet kuṭilayā sūcyā mudga-mātrāntaraiḥ padaiḥ ।।

baddhvā lalāṭe paṭṭaṃ ca tatra sīvana-sūtrakam ।
nāti-gāḍha-ślathaṃ sūcyā nikṣiped atha yojayet ।।

madhu-sarpiḥ-kavalikāṃ na cāsmin bandham ācaret ।
nyagrodhādi-kaṣāyaiś ca sa-kṣīraiḥ secayed ruji ।।

pañcame divase sūtram apanīyāvacūrṇayet ।
gairikeṇa vraṇaṃ yuñjyāt tīkṣṇaṃ nasyāñjanādi ca ।।

īkṣṇa-nasyāñjanādi ca īkṣṇa-nasyāñjanāni ca 
tīkṣṇaṃ nasyāñjanāni ca
dahed a-śāntau nirbhujya vartma-doṣāśrayāṃ valīm ।
saṃdaṃśenādhikaṃ pakṣma hṛtvā tasyāśrayaṃ dahet ।।

sūcy-agreṇāgni-varṇena dāho bāhyālajeḥ punaḥ ।
bhinnasya kṣāra-vahnibhyāṃ su-cchinnasyārbudasya ca ।।

uttarasthāna
vāyuḥ kruddhaḥ sirāḥ prāpya jalābhaṃ jala-vāhinīḥ ।
aśru srāvayate vartma-śukla-saṃdheḥ kanīnakāt ।।

-śukla-saṃdhi-kanīnikāt
tena netraṃ sa-rug-rāga-śophaṃ syāt sa jalāsravaḥ ।
kaphāt kaphāsrave śvetaṃ picchilaṃ bahalaṃ sravet ।।

aphāt kapha-śrave śvetaṃ aphāt kapha-srave śvetaṃ
kaphena śophas tīkṣṇāgraḥ kṣāra-budbudakopamaḥ ।
pṛthu-mūla-balaḥ snigdhaḥ sa-varṇo mṛdu-picchilaḥ ।।

a-varṇa-mṛdu-picchilaḥ
mahān a-pākaḥ kaṇḍū-mān upanāhaḥ sa nī-rujaḥ ।
raktād raktāsrāve tāmraṃ bahūṣṇaṃ cāśru saṃsravet ।।

aktād rakta-srave tāmraṃ aktād raktaṃ sravet tāmraṃ 
bahūṣṇaṃ vāśru saṃsravet
vartma-saṃdhy-āśrayā śukle piṭikā dāha-śūlinī ।
tāmrā mudgopamā bhinnā raktaṃ sravati parvaṇī ।।

pūyāsrave malāḥ sāsrā vartma-saṃdheḥ kanīnakāt ।
srāvayanti muhuḥ pūyaṃ sāsraṃ tvaṅ-māṃsa-pākataḥ ।।

artma-saṃdhi-kanīnakāt āsra-tvaṅ-māṃsa-pākataḥ 
sāśru-tvaṅ-māṃsa-pākataḥ
pūyālaso vraṇaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śopha-saṃrambha-pūrvakaḥ ।
kanīna-saṃdhāv ādhmāyī pūyāsrāvī sa-vedanaḥ ।।

kanīnasyāntar alajī śopho ruk-toda-dāha-vān ।
apāṅge vā kanīne vā kaṇḍūṣā-pakṣma-poṭa-vān ।।

pūyāsrāvī kṛmi-granthir granthiḥ kṛmi-yuto arti-mān ।
upanāha-kṛmi-granthi-pūyālasaka-parvaṇīḥ ।।

śastreṇa sādhayet pañca sālajīn āsravāṃs tyajet ।
pittaṃ kuryāt site bindūn asita-śyāva-pītakān ।।

malāktādarśa-tulyaṃ vā sarvaṃ śuklaṃ sa-dāha-ruk ।
rogo ayaṃ śuktikā-saṃjñaḥ sa-śakṛd-bheda-tṛḍ-jvaraḥ ।।

arvaṃ śuklam a-dāha-ruk
kaphāc chukle samaṃ śvetaṃ cira-vṛddhy-adhi-māṃsakam ।
śuklārma śophas tv a-rujaḥ sa-varṇo bahalo a-mṛduḥ ।।

guruḥ snigdho ambu-bindv-ābho balāsa-grathitaṃ smṛtaṃ ।
bindubhiḥ piṣṭa-dhavalair utsannaiḥ piṣṭakaṃ vadet ।।

alāsa-granthi sa smṛtaḥ
rakta-rājī-tataṃ śuklam uṣyate yat sa-vedanam ।
a-śophāśrūpadehaṃ ca sirotpātaḥ sa śoṇitāt ।।

a-śothāśrūpadehaṃ ca
upekṣitah sirotpāto rājīs tā eva vardhayan ।
kuryāt sāsraṃ sirā-harṣaṃ tenākṣy-udvīkṣaṇā-kṣamam ।।

uryāt sāśruṃ sirā-harṣaṃ enākṣaṃ vīkṣaṇā-kṣamam
sirā-jāle sirā-jālaṃ bṛhad raktaṃ ghanonnatam ।
śoṇitārma samaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ padmābham adhi-māṃsakam ।।

nī-ruk ślakṣṇo arjunaṃ binduḥ śaśa-lohita-lohitaḥ ।
mṛdv-āśu-vṛddhy-a-ruṅ-māṃsaṃ prastāri śyāva-lohitam ।।

prastāry-arma malaiḥ sāsraiḥ snāvārma snāva-saṃnibham ।
śuṣkāsṛk-piṇḍa-vac chyāvaṃ yan māṃsaṃ bahalaṃ pṛthu ।।

adhi-māṃsārma tad dāha-gharṣa-vatyaḥ sirāvṛtāḥ ।
kṛṣṇāsannāḥ sirā-saṃjñāḥ piṭikāḥ sarṣapopamāḥ ।।

dhi-māṃsārma rug-dāha-
śukti-harṣa-sirotpāta-piṣṭaka-grathitārjunam ।
sādhayed auṣadhaiḥ ṣaṭkaṃ śeṣaṃ śastreṇa saptakam ।।

śukti-harṣa-sirotpātān iṣṭaka-grathitārjunam
navotthaṃ tad api dravyair armoktaṃ yac ca pañca-dhā ।
tac chedyam asita-prāptaṃ māṃsa-snāva-sirāvṛtam ।।

rmoktaṃ yat tu pañca-dhā
carmoddāla-vad ucchrāyi dṛṣṭi-prāptaṃ ca varjayet ।
pittaṃ kṛṣṇe atha-vā dṛṣṭau śukraṃ todāśru-rāga-vat ।।

ṛṣṭi-prāptaṃ tu varjayet śukraṃ todāsra-rāga-vat
chittvā tvacaṃ janayati tena syāt kṛṣṇa-maṇḍalam ।
pakva-jambū-nibhaṃ kiñ-cin nimnaṃ ca kṣata-śukrakam ।।

tat kṛcchra-sādhyaṃ yāpyaṃ tu dvitīya-paṭala-vyadhāt ।
tatra todādi-bāhulyaṃ sūcī-viddhābha-kṛṣṇa-tā ।।

tṛtīya-paṭala-cchedād a-sādhyaṃ nicitaṃ vraṇaiḥ ।
śaṅkha-śuklaṃ kaphāt sādhyaṃ nāti-ruk śuddha-śukrakam ।।

ā-tāmra-picchilāsra-srud ā-tāmra-piṭikāti-ruk ।
ajā-viṭ-sadṛśocchrāya-kārṣṇyā varjyāsṛjājakā ।।

ā-tāmra-picchilāśruḥ syād ā-tāmra-picchilāsṛk syād jā-viṭ-sadṛśocchrāyā 
ṛṣṇā varjyāsṛjājakā
sirā-śukraṃ malaiḥ sāsrais taj-juṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇa-maṇḍalam ।
sa-toda-dāha-tāmrābhiḥ sirābhir avatanyate ।।

a-nimittoṣṇa-śītāccha-ghanāsra-sruc ca tat tyajet ।
doṣaiḥ sāsraiḥ sakṛt kṛṣṇaṃ nīyate śukla-rūpa-tām ।।

-ghanāśru syāc ca tat tyajet -ghanāśru-srāvi tat tyajet c -ghanāśru-sruc ca tat tyajet 
oṣaiḥ sāsraiḥ sa-dṛk kṛṣṇaṃ
dhavalābhropaliptābhaṃ niṣpāvārdha-dalākṛti ।
ati-tīvra-rujā-rāga-dāha-śvayathu-pīḍitam ।।

pākātyayena tac chukraṃ varjayet tīvra-vedanam ।
yasya vā liṅga-nāśo antaḥ śyāvaṃ yad vā sa-lohitam ।।

aty-utsedhāvagāḍhaṃ vā sāśru nāḍī-vraṇāvṛtam ।
purāṇaṃ viṣamaṃ madhye vicchinnaṃ yac ca śukrakam ।।

āsra-nāḍī-vraṇāvṛtam pañcety uktā gadāḥ kṛṣṇe sādhyā-sādhya-vibhāgataḥ ।।

uttarasthāna
upanāhaṃ bhiṣak svinnaṃ bhinnaṃ vrīhi-mukhena ca ।
lekhayen maṇḍalāgreṇa tataś ca pratisārayet ।।

hinnaṃ vrīhi-mukhena tu
pippalī-kṣaudra-sindhūtthair badhnīyāt pūrva-vat tataḥ ।
paṭola-pattrāmalaka-kvāthenāścyotayec ca tam ।।

parvaṇī baḍiśenāttā bāhya-saṃdhi-tri-bhāgataḥ ।
vṛddhi-pattreṇa vardhyārdhe syād aśru-gatir anya-thā ।।

arvaṇī baḍiśenāntar- -bāhya-saṃdhi-tri-bhāgataḥ yād asra-gatir anya-thā 
yād asra-srutir anya-thā
cikitsā cārma-vat kṣaudra-saindhava-pratisāritā ।
pūyālase sirāṃ vidhyet tatas tam upanāhayet ।।

atas tad upanāhayet
kurvīta cākṣi-pākoktaṃ sarvaṃ karma yathā-vidhi ।
saindhavārdraka-kāsīsa-loha-tāmraiḥ su-cūrṇitaiḥ ।।

cūrṇāñjanaṃ prayuñjīta sa-kṣaudrair vā rasa-kriyām ।
kṛmi-granthiṃ karīṣeṇa svinnaṃ bhittvā vilikhya ca ।।

tri-phalā-kṣaudra-kāsīsa-saindhavaiḥ pratisārayet ।
pittābhiṣyanda-vac chuktiṃ balāsāhvaya-piṣṭake ।।

alāsāhvaya-piṣṭakau
kaphābhiṣyanda-van muktvā sirā-vyadham upācaret ।
bījapūra-rasāktaṃ ca vyoṣa-kaṭphalam añjanam ।।

jātī-mukula-sindhūttha-devadāru-mahauṣadhaiḥ ।
piṣṭaiḥ prasannayā vartiḥ śopha-kaṇḍū-ghnam añjanam ।।

śopha-kaṇḍū-ghnam auṣadham
rakta-syanda-vad utpāta-harṣa-jālārjuna-kriyā ।
sirotpāte viśeṣeṇa ghṛta-mākṣikam añjanam ।।

sirā-harṣe tu madhunā ślakṣṇa-ghṛṣṭaṃ rasāñjanam ।
arjune śarkarā-mastu-kṣaudrair āścyotanaṃ hitam ।।

sphaṭikaḥ kuṅkumaṃ śaṅkho madhukaṃ madhunāñjanam ।
madhunā cāñjanaṃ śaṅkhaḥ pheno vā sitayā saha ।।

phaṭikaṃ kuṅkumaṃ śaṅkhaṃ āsīsaṃ madhunāñjanam
armoktaṃ pañca-dhā tatra tanu dhūmāvilaṃ ca yat ।
raktaṃ dadhi-nibhaṃ yac ca śukra-vat tasya bheṣajam ।।

uttānasyetarat svinnaṃ sa-sindhūtthena cāñjitam ।
rasena bījapūrasya nimīlyākṣi vimardayet ।।

itthaṃ saṃroṣitākṣasya pracale armādhi-māṃsake ।
ghṛtasya niś-calaṃ mūrdhni vartmanoś ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

rabale armādhi-māṃsake
apāṅgam īkṣamāṇasya vṛddhe armaṇi kanīnakāt ।
valī syād yatra tatrārma baḍiśenāvalambitam ।।

nāty-āyataṃ mucuṇḍyā vā sūcyā sūtreṇa vā tataḥ ।
samantān maṇḍalāgreṇa mocayed atha mokṣitam ।।

āty-āyataṃ samutpāṭya
kanīnakam upānīya catur-bhāgāvaśeṣitam ।
chindyāt kanīnakaṃ rakṣed vāhinīś cāśru-vāhinīḥ ।।

hindyāt kanīnakaṃ rakṣan hindyāt kanīnakaṃ rakṣye
kanīnaka-vyadhād aśru nāḍī cākṣṇi pravartate ।
vṛddhe armaṇi tathāpāṅgāt paśyato asya kanīnakam ।।

anīnaka-vadhād aśru anīnaka-vadhād āśu anīnaka-vyadhād a-sru- 
-nāḍī cākṣṇi pravartate
samyak-chinnaṃ madhu-vyoṣa-saindhava-pratisāritam ।
uṣṇena sarpiṣā siktam abhyaktaṃ madhu-sarpiṣā ।।

badhnīyāt secayen muktvā tṛtīyādi-dineṣu ca ।
karañja-bīja-siddhena kṣīreṇa kvathitais tathā ।।

sa-kṣaudrair dvi-niśā-lodhra-paṭolī-yaṣṭi-kiṃśukaiḥ ।
kuraṇṭa-mukulopetair muñced evāhni saptame ।।

oraṇṭa-mukulopetair
samyak-chinne bhavet svāsthyaṃ hīnāti-ccheda-jān gadān ।
sekāñjana-prabhṛtibhir jayel lekhana-bṛṃhaṇaiḥ ।।

sitā-manaḥśilaileya-lavaṇottama-nāgaram ।
ardha-karṣonmitaṃ tārkṣyaṃ palārdhaṃ ca madhu-drutam ।।

alārdhaṃ ca madhu-plutam
añjanaṃ śleṣma-timira-pilla-śukrārma-śoṣa-jit ।
tri-phalaika-tama-dravya-tvacaṃ pānīya-kalkitām ।।

-pilla-śukrārma-kāca-jit
śarāva-pihitāṃ dagdhvā kapāle cūrṇayet tataḥ ।
pṛthak-śeṣauṣadha-rasaiḥ pṛthag eva ca bhāvitā ।।

sā maṣī śoṣitā peṣyā bhūyo dvi-lavaṇānvitā ।
trīṇy etāny añjanāny āha lekhanāni paraṃ nimiḥ ।।

sirā-jāle sirā yās tu kaṭhinā lekhanauṣadhaiḥ ।
na sidhyanty arma-vat tāsāṃ piṭikānāṃ ca sādhanam ।।

doṣānurodhāc chukreṣu snigdha-rūkṣā varā ghṛtam ।
tiktam ūrdhvam asṛk-srāvo reka-sekādi ceṣyate ।।

oṣānubandhāc chukreṣu nigdhā rūkṣā varā ghṛtam nigdha-rūkṣa-varā ghṛtam 
iktam ūrdhvam asṛk-srāva- -reka-sekādi ceṣyate
tris trivṛd-vāriṇā pakvaṃ kṣata-śukre ghṛtaṃ pibet ।
sirayānu hared raktaṃ jalaukobhiś ca locanāt ।।

siddhenotpala-kākolī-drākṣā-yaṣṭī-vidāribhiḥ ।
sa-sitenāja-payasā secanaṃ salilena vā ।।

rāgāśru-vedanā-śāntau paraṃ lekhanam añjanam ।
vartayo jāti-mukula-lākṣā-gairika-candanaiḥ ।।

prasādayanti pittāsraṃ ghnanti ca kṣata-śukrakam ।
dantair danti-varāhoṣṭra-gavāśvāja-kharodbhavaiḥ ।।

rasādayanti pittāsṛk -go-rāsabha-samudbhavaiḥ
sa-śaṅkha-mauktikāmbho-dhi-phenair marica-pādikaiḥ ।
kṣata-śukram api vyāpi danta-vartir nivartayet ।।

tamāla-pattraṃ go-danta-śaṅkha-pheno asthi gārdabham ।
tāmraṃ ca vartir mūtreṇa sarva-śukraka-nāśinī ।।

āmraṃ ca basta-mūtreṇa
ratnāni dantāḥ śṛṅgāṇi dhātavas try-ūṣaṇaṃ truṭī ।
karañja-bījaṃ laśuno vraṇa-sādi ca bheṣajam ।।

sa-vraṇā-vraṇa-gambhīra-tvak-stha-śukra-ghnam añjanam ।
nimnam unnamayet sneha-pāna-nasya-rasāñjanaiḥ ।।

sa-rujaṃ nī-rujaṃ tṛpti-puṭa-pākena śukrakam ।
śuddha-śukre niśā-yaṣṭī-śārivā-śābarāmbhasā ।।

-śārivā-sādhitāmbhasā
secanaṃ lodhra-poṭalyā koṣṇāmbho-magnayātha-vā ।
bṛhatī-mūla-yaṣṭy-āhva-tāmra-saindhava-nāgaraiḥ ।।

dhātrī-phalāmbunā piṣṭair lepitaṃ tāmra-bhājanam ।
yavājyāmalakī-pattrair bahu-śo dhūpayet tataḥ ।।

tatra kurvīta guṭikās tā jala-kṣaudra-peṣitāḥ ।
mahā-nīlā iti khyātāḥ śuddha-śukra-harāḥ param ।।

sthire śukre ghane cāsya bahu-śo apahared asṛk ।
śiraḥ-kāya-virekāṃś ca puṭa-pākāṃś ca bhūri-śaḥ ।।

kuryān marica-vaidehī-śirīṣa-phala-saindhavaiḥ ।
harṣaṇaṃ tri-phalā-kvātha-pītena lavaṇena vā ।।

harṣaṇaṃ tri-phalā-kvātha- arṣapa-tri-phalā-kvātha-
kuryād añjana-yogau vā ślokārdha-gaditāv imau ।
śaṅkha-kolāsthi-kataka-drākṣā-madhuka-mākṣikaiḥ ।।

surā-dantārṇava-malaiḥ śirīṣa-kusumānvitaiḥ ।
dhātrī-phaṇijjaka-rase kṣāro lāṅgalikodbhavaḥ ।।

hara-dantārṇava-malaiḥ ṣāro lāṅgalikā-bhavaḥ 
kṣāro lāṅgalikī-bhavaḥ
uṣitaḥ śoṣitaś cūrṇaḥ śukra-harṣaṇam añjanam ।
mudgā vā nis-tuṣāḥ piṣṭāḥ śaṅkha-kṣaudra-samāyutāḥ ।।

śukra-gharṣaṇam añjanam
sāro madhūkān madhu-mān majjā vākṣāt sa-mākṣikā ।
go-kharāśvoṣṭra-daśanāḥ śaṅkhaḥ phenaḥ samudra-jaḥ ।।

āro madhūkāt sa-madhur āro madhūkān madhunā
vartir arjuna-toyena hṛṣṭa-śukraka-nāśinī ।
utsannaṃ vā sa-śalyaṃ vā śūkraṃ vālādibhir likhet ।।

iṣṭā śukraka-nāśinī uṣṭa-śukraka-nāśinī
sirā-śukre tv a-dṛṣṭi-ghne cikitsā vraṇa-śukra-vat ।
puṇḍra-yaṣṭy-āhva-kākolī-siṃhī-loha-niśāñjanam ।।

kalkitaṃ chāga-dugdhena sa-ghṛtair dhūpitaṃ yavaiḥ ।
dhātrī-pattraiś ca paryāyād vartir atrāñjanaṃ param ।।

artir atrāñjanaṃ hitam artir netrāñjanaṃ param
a-śāntāv arma-vac chastram ajakākhye ca yojayet ।
ajakāyām a-sādhyāyāṃ śukre anya-tra ca tad-vidhe ।।

vedanopaśamaṃ sneha-pānāsṛk-srāvaṇādibhiḥ ।
kuryād bībhatsa-tāṃ jetuṃ śukrasyotsedha-sādhanam ।।

śukla-tvotsedha-sādhanam
nārikelāsthi-bhallāta-tāla-vaṃśa-karīra-jam ।
bhasmādbhiḥ srāvayet tābhir bhāvayet karabhāsthi-jam ।।

cūrṇaṃ śukreṣv a-sādhyeṣu tad vaivarṇya-ghnam añjanam ।
sādhyeṣu sādhanāyālam idam eva ca śīlitam ।।

ajakāṃ pārśvato viddhvā sūcyā visrāvya codakam ।
samaṃ prapīḍyāṅguṣṭhena vasārdreṇānu pūrayet ।।

vraṇaṃ go-māṃsa-cūrṇena baddhaṃ baddhaṃ vimucya ca ।
sapta-rātrād vraṇe rūḍhe kṛṣṇa-bhāge same sthire ।।

snehāñjanaṃ ca kartavyaṃ nasyaṃ ca kṣīra-sarpiṣā ।
tathāpi punar-ādhmāne bheda-cchedādikāṃ kriyām ।।

athāpi punar-ādhmāte yuktyā kuryād yathā nāti-cchedena syāt nimajjanam ।।

ū̆yuktyā yuñjyād yathā nāti-
nityaṃ ca śukreṣu śṛtaṃ yathā-svaṃ pāne ca marśe ca ghṛtaṃ vidadhyāt ।
na hīyate labdha-balā tathāntas tīkṣṇāñjanair dṛk satataṃ prayuktaiḥ ।।

īkṣṇāñjanair dṛk pratataṃ prayuktaiḥ

uttarasthāna
sirānusāriṇi male prathamaṃ paṭalaṃ śrite ।
a-vyaktam īkṣate rūpaṃ vyaktam apy a-nimittataḥ ।।

rathamaṃ paṭalaṃ gate -vyaktam īkṣyate rūpaṃ
prāpte dvitīyaṃ paṭalaṃ a-bhūtam api paśyati ।
bhūtaṃ tu yatnād āsannaṃ dūre sūkṣmaṃ ca nekṣate ।।

ūraṃ sūkṣmaṃ ca nekṣate
dūrāntika-sthaṃ rūpaṃ ca viparyāsena manyate ।
doṣe maṇḍala-saṃsthāne maṇḍalānīva paśyati ।।

dvi-dhaikaṃ dṛṣṭi-madhya-sthe bahu-dhā bahu-dhā-sthite ।
dṛṣṭer abhyantara-gate hrasva-vṛddha-viparyayam ।।

rasva-dīrgha-viparyayam rasvaṃ bahu viparyayam
nāntika-stham adhaḥ-saṃsthe dūra-gaṃ nopari sthite ।
pārśve paśyen na pārśva-sthe timirākhyo ayam āmayaḥ ।।

prāpnoti kāca-tāṃ doṣe tṛtīya-paṭalāśrite ।
tenordhvam īkṣate nādhas tanu-cailāvṛtopamam ।।

enordhvam īkṣyate nādhas
yathā-varṇaṃ ca rajyeta dṛṣṭir hīyeta ca kramāt ।
tathāpy upekṣamāṇasya caturthaṃ paṭalaṃ gataḥ ।।

athā-doṣaṃ ca rajyeta
liṅga-nāśaṃ malaḥ kurvaṃś chādayed dṛṣṭi-maṇḍalam ।
tatra vātena timire vyāviddham iva paśyati ।।

calāvilāruṇābhāsaṃ prasannaṃ cekṣate muhuḥ ।
jālāni keśān maśakān raśmīṃś copekṣite atra ca ।।

hūmāvilāruṇābhāsaṃ rasannaṃ vīkṣate muhuḥ 
raśmīṃś copekṣite atra tu
kācī-bhūte dṛg aruṇā paśyaty āsyam a-nāsikam ।
candra-dīpādy-aneka-tvaṃ vakram ṛjv api manyate ।।

vṛddhaḥ kāco dṛśaṃ kuryād rajo-dhūmāvṛtām iva ।
spaṣṭāruṇābhāṃ vistīrṇāṃ sūkṣmāṃ vā hata-darśanām ।।

phuṭāruṇābhāṃ vistīrṇāṃ
sa liṅga-nāśo vāte tu saṃkocayati dṛk-sirāḥ ।
dṛṅ-maṇḍalaṃ viśaty antar gambhīrā dṛg asau smṛtā ।।

pitta-je timire vidyut-khadyota-dyota-dīpitam ।
śikhi-tittiri-pattrābhaṃ prāyo nīlaṃ ca paśyati ।।

-khadyotodyota-dīpitam śikhi-tittiri-picchābhaṃ
kāce dṛg kāca-nīlābhā tādṛg eva ca paśyati ।
arkendu-pariveṣāgni-marīcīndra-dhanūṃṣi ca ।।

āce dṛg kāṃsya-nīlābhā
bhṛṅga-nīlā nir-ālokā dṛk snigdhā liṅga-nāśataḥ ।
dṛṣṭiḥ pittena hrasvākhyā sā hrasvā hrasva-darśinī ।।

bhavet pitta-vidagdhākhyā pītā pītābha-darśanā ।
kaphena timire prāyaḥ snigdhaṃ śvetaṃ ca paśyati ।।

ītā pītābha-darśinī
śaṅkhendu-kunda-kusumaiḥ kumudair iva cācitam ।
kāce tu niṣ-prabhendv-arka-pradīpādyair ivācitam ।।

umudair iva vācitam
sitābhā sā ca dṛṣṭiḥ syāl liṅga-nāśe tu lakṣyate ।
mūrtaḥ kapho dṛṣṭi-gataḥ snigdho darśana-nāśanaḥ ।।

bindur jalasyeva calaḥ padminī-puṭa-saṃsthitaḥ ।
uṣṇe saṃkocam āyāti cchāyāyāṃ parisarpati ।।

adminī-puṭa-saṃśritaḥ adminī-pattra-saṃśritaḥ
śaṅkha-kundendu-kumuda-sphaṭikopama-śuklimā ।
raktena timire raktaṃ tamo-bhūtaṃ ca paśyati ।।

kācena raktā kṛṣṇā vā dṛṣṭis tādṛk ca paśyati ।
liṅga-nāśe api tādṛg dṛṅ niṣ-prabhā hata-darśanā ।।

saṃsarga-saṃnipāteṣu vidyāt saṃkīrṇa-lakṣaṇān ।
timirādīn a-kasmāc ca taiḥ syād vyaktākulekṣaṇaḥ ।।

aiḥ syād vakrākulekṣaṇaḥ aiḥ syād vyaktākulekṣaṇam
timire śeṣayor dṛṣṭau citro rāgaḥ prajāyate ।
dyotyate nakulasyeva yasya dṛṅ nicitā malaiḥ ।।

nakulāndhaḥ sa tatrāhni citraṃ paśyati no niśi ।
arke asta-mastaka-nyasta-gabhastau stambham āgatāḥ ।।

sthagayanti dṛśaṃ doṣā doṣāndhaḥ sa gado aparaḥ ।
divā-kara-kara-spṛṣṭā bhraṣṭā dṛṣṭi-pathān malāḥ ।।

vilīna-līnā yacchanti vyaktam atrāhni darśanam ।
uṣṇa-taptasya sahasā śīta-vāri-nimajjanāt ।।

tri-doṣa-rakta-saṃpṛkto yāty ūṣmordhvaṃ tato akṣiṇi ।
dāhoṣe malinaṃ śuklam ahany āvila-darśanam ।।

rātrāv āndhyaṃ ca jāyeta vidagdhoṣṇena sā smṛtā ।
bhṛśam amlāśanād doṣaiḥ sāsrair yā dṛṣṭir ācitā ।।

sa-kleda-kaṇḍū-kaluṣā vidagdhāmlena sā smṛtā ।
śoka-jvara-śiro-roga-saṃtaptasyānilādayaḥ ।।

idagdhāmlena sā matā
dhūmāvilāṃ dhūma-dṛśaṃ dṛśaṃ kuryuḥ sa dhūmaraḥ ।
sahasaivālpa-sat-tvasya paśyato rūpam adbhutam ।।

hūmāvilāṃ dhūma-dṛśāṃ ṛśaṃ kuryuḥ sa dhūsaraḥ 
dṛśaṃ kuryuḥ sa dhūmakaḥ
bhāsvaraṃ bhās-karādiṃ vā vātādyā nayanāśritāḥ ।
kurvanti tejaḥ saṃśoṣya dṛṣṭiṃ muṣita-darśanām ।।

hāsuraṃ bhās-karādiṃ vā
vaiḍūrya-varṇāṃ stimitāṃ prakṛti-sthām ivā-vyathām ।
aupasargika ity eṣa liṅga-nāśo atra varjayet ।।

vinā kaphāl liṅga-nāśān gambhīrāṃ hrasva-jām api ।
ṣaṭ kācā nakulāndhaś ca yāpyāḥ śeṣāṃs tu sādhayet ।।

ṣaṭ kācā nakulāndhyaś ca dvā-daśeti gadā dṛṣṭau nirdiṣṭāḥ sapta-viṃśatiḥ ।।

uttarasthāna
timiraṃ kāca-tāṃ yāti kāco apy āndhyam upekṣayā ।
netra-rogeṣv ato ghoraṃ timiraṃ sādhayed drutam ।।

tulāṃ paceta jīvantyā droṇe apāṃ pāda-śeṣite ।
tat-kvāthe dvi-guṇa-kṣīraṃ ghṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।।

at-kvāthe dvi-guṇaṃ kṣīraṃ
prapauṇḍarīka-kākolī-pippalī-lodhra-saindhavaiḥ ।
śatāhvā-madhuka-drākṣā-sitā-dāru-phala-trayaiḥ ।।

kārṣikair niśi tat pītaṃ timirāpaharaṃ param ।
drākṣā-candana-mañjiṣṭhā-kākolī-dvaya-jīvakaiḥ ।।

imirāṇāṃ haraṃ param
sitā-śatāvarī-medā-puṇḍrāhva-madhukotpalaiḥ ।
pacej jīrṇa-ghṛta-prasthaṃ sama-kṣīraṃ picūnmitaiḥ ।।

acej jīrṇaṃ ghṛta-prasthaṃ
hanti tat kāca-timira-rakta-rājī-śiro-rujaḥ ।
paṭola-nimba-kaṭukā-dārvī-sevya-varā-vṛṣam ।।

sa-dhanvayāsa-trāyantī-parpaṭaṃ pālikaṃ pṛthak ।
prastham āmalakānāṃ ca kvāthayen nalvaṇe ambhasi ।।

tad-āḍhake ardha-palikaiḥ piṣṭaiḥ prasthaṃ ghṛtāt pacet ।
musta-bhūnimba-yaṣṭy-āhva-kuṭajodīcya-candanaiḥ ।।

ad-āḍhake ardha-palikair hṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet
sa-pippalīkais tat sarpir ghrāṇa-karṇāsya-roga-jit ।
vidradhi-jvara-duṣṭārur-visarpāpaci-kuṣṭha-nut ।।

a-vyoṣa-cavyais tat sarpir hrāṇa-karṇākṣi-roga-jit 
vidradhi-jvara-duṣṭāsra-
viśeṣāc chukra-timira-naktāndhyoṣṇāmla-dāha-hṛt ।
tri-phalāṣṭa-palaṃ kvāthyaṃ pāda-śeṣaṃ jalāḍhake ।।

-naktāndhyoṣṇāmla-dāha-nut āda-śeṣe jalāḍhake
tena tulya-payaskena tri-phalā-pala-kalka-vān ।
ardha-prastho ghṛtāt siddhaḥ sitayā mākṣikeṇa vā ।।

yuktaṃ pibet tat timirī tad-yuktaṃ vā varā-rasam ।
yaṣṭīmadhu-dvi-kākolī-vyāghrī-kṛṣṇāmṛtotpalaiḥ ।।

pālikaiḥ sa-sitā-drākṣair ghṛta-prasthaṃ pacet samaiḥ ।
ajā-kṣīra-varā-vasā-mārkava-sva-rasaiḥ pṛthak ।।

mahā-traiphalam ity etat paraṃ dṛṣṭi-vikāra-jit ।
traiphalenātha haviṣā lihānas tri-phalāṃ niśi ।।

araṃ dṛṣṭi-vikāra-nut
yaṣṭīmadhuka-saṃyuktāṃ madhunā ca pariplutām ।
māsam ekaṃ hitāhāraḥ pibann āmalakodakam ।।

sauparṇaṃ labhate cakṣur ity āha bhaga-vān nimiḥ ।
tāpyāyo-hema-yaṣṭy-āhva-sitā-jīrṇājya-mākṣikaiḥ ।।

saṃyojitā yathā-kāmaṃ timira-ghnī varā varā ।
sa-ghṛtaṃ vā varā-kvāthaṃ śīlayet timirāmayī ।।

apūpa-sūpa-saktūn vā tri-phalā-cūrṇa-saṃyutān ।
pāyasaṃ vā varā-yuktaṃ śītaṃ sa-madhu-śarkaram ।।

pūpa-takra-saktūn vā
prātar bhaktasya vā pūrvam adyāt pathyāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।
mṛdvīkā-śarkarā-kṣaudraiḥ satataṃ timirāturaḥ ।।

rātar bhuktasya vā pūrvam
sroto-jāṃśāṃś catuḥ-ṣaṣṭiṃ tāmrāyo-rūpya-kāñcanaiḥ ।
yuktān praty-ekam ekāṃśair andha-mūṣodara-sthitān ।।

dhmāpayitvā samāvṛttaṃ tatas tac ca niṣecayet ।
rasa-skandha-kaṣāyeṣu sapta-kṛtvaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।।

vaiḍūrya-muktā-śaṅkhānāṃ tribhir bhāgair yutaṃ tataḥ ।
cūrṇāñjanaṃ prayuñjīta tat sarva-timirāpaham ।।

at sarvaṃ timirāpaham
māṃsī-tri-jātakāyaḥ-kuṅkuma-nīlotpalābhayā-tutthaiḥ ।
sita-kāca-śaṅkha-phenaka-maricāñjana-pippalī-madhukaiḥ ।।

candre aśvinī-sa-nāthe su-cūrṇitair añjayed yugalaṃ akṣṇoḥ ।
timirārma-rakta-rājī-kaṇḍū-kācādi-śamam icchan ।।

marica-vara-lavaṇa-bhāgau bhāgau dvau kaṇa-samudra-phenābhyām ।
sauvīra-bhāga-navakaṃ citrāyāṃ cūrṇitaṃ kaphāmaya-jit ।।

itrā-saṃcūrṇitaṃ kaphāmaya-jit
manohvā-tuttha-kastūrī-māṃsī-malaya-rocanāḥ ।
daśa-karpūra-saṃyuktam aśīti-guṇam añjanam ।।

dara-karpūra-saṃyuktam
piṣṭaṃ citrāśvinī-puṣye ṣaḍ-vidhe timire hitam ।
prasādanaṃ ca dṛṣṭeḥ syāc cakṣuṣeṇāvabhāṣitam ।।

drākṣā-mṛṇālī-sva-rase kṣīra-madya-vasāsu ca ।
pṛthak divyāpsu sroto-jaṃ sapta-kṛtvo niṣecayet ।।

tac cūrṇitaṃ sthitaṃ śaṅkhe dṛk-prasādanam añjanam ।
śastaṃ sarvākṣi-rogeṣu videha-pati-nirmitam ।।

ac cūrṇitaṃ ghṛtaṃ śaṅkhe
nirdagdhaṃ bādarāṅgārais tutthaṃ cetthaṃ niṣecitam ।
kramād ajā-payaḥ-sarpiḥ-kṣaudre tasmāt pala-dvayam ।।

utthaṃ caivaṃ niṣecitam ramāc chāga-payaḥ-sarpiḥ-
kārṣikais tāpya-marica-sroto-ja-kaṭukā-nataiḥ ।
paṭu-lodhra-śilā-pathyā-kaṇailāñjana-phenakaiḥ ।।

yuktaṃ palena yaṣṭyāś ca mūṣāntar-dhmāta-cūrṇitam ।
hanti kācārma-naktāndhya-rakta-rājīḥ su-śīlitaḥ ।।

cūrṇo viśeṣāt timiraṃ bhās-karo bhās-karo yathā ।
triṃśad-bhāgā bhujaṅgasya gandha-pāṣāṇa-pañcakam ।।

śulba-tālakayor dvau dvau vaṅgasyaiko añjanāt trayam ।
andha-mūṣī-kṛtaṃ dhmātaṃ pakvaṃ vi-malam añjanam ।।

śulba-tārakayor dvau dvau ndha-mūṣā-gataṃ dhmātaṃ timirānta-karaṃ loke dvitīya iva bhās-karaḥ ।।

imirāpaharaṃ loke go-mūtre chagaṇa-rase amla-kāñjike ca strī-stanye ।।

o-mūtre chagala-rase amla-kāñjike ca haviṣi viṣe ca mākṣike ca ।।
yat tutthaṃ jvalitam aneka-śo niṣiktaṃ ।।tat kuryād garuḍa-samaṃ narasya cakṣuḥ ।।
tutthaṃ sa-kāśaṃ kanakaṃ sa-phalaṃ śaṅkha-śilā-gairikam añjanaṃ ca ।
naraḥ kapāla-sahi-kūṅkuḍāṇḍaṃ sapta-dvi-sapta-tri-samayo gataḥ ।।

bhṛṅgodbhava-sva-rasa-bhāvitam āja-dugdhe mūtre gavām payasi ca tri-phalā-kaṣāye ।
drākṣā-rase ca pariśuddham iti krameṇa sauvīram añjanam idaṃ timiraṃ nihanti ।। 

।।

śreṣṭhā-jalaṃ bhṛṅga-rasaṃ sa-viṣājyam ajā-payaḥ ।
yaṣṭī-rasaṃ ca yat sīsaṃ sapta-kṛtvaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।।

śreṣṭhā-rasaṃ bhṛṅga-rasaṃ
taptaṃ taptaṃ pāyitaṃ tac-chalākā netre yuktā sāñjanān-añjanā vā ।
taimiryārma-srāva-paicchilya-paillaṃ kaṇḍūṃ jāḍyaṃ rakta-rājīṃ ca hanti ।।

rasendra-bhujagau tulyau tayos tulyam athāñjanam ।
īṣat-karpūra-saṃyuktam añjanaṃ timirāpaham ।।

īṣat-karpūra-sahitam ñjanaṃ timire varam ñjanaṃ 
nayanāmṛtam
yo gṛdhras taruṇa-ravi-prakāśa-gallas tasyāsyaṃ samaya-mṛtasya go-śakṛdbhiḥ ।
nirdagdhaṃ sama-ghṛtam añjanaṃ ca peṣyaṃ yogo ayaṃ nayana-balaṃ karoti gārdhram ।। 
।।

kṛṣṇa-sarpa-vadane sa-haviṣkaṃ dagdham añjana-niḥsṛta-dhūmam ।
cūrṇitaṃ nalada-pattra-vimiśraṃ bhinna-tāram api rakṣati cakṣuḥ ।।

agdham añjana-nirgata-dhūmam ojitaṃ nalada-pattra-vimiśraṃ
nāgāñjanāśmāla-śilārka-vaṅgais triṃśad-dvi-pañca-dvayam a-dvikaikaiḥ ।
andha-mūṣī-kṛtaiś chāga-payo-niṣiktair dṛṣṭer idaṃ bhās-karam añjanaṃ syāt ।।

sroto-'śma-vīraṃ veṣṭyājamodā-vaṭa-cchadaiḥ ।
ṣaṭkaṃ timira-jit kliṣṭaṃ mṛl-liptaṃ go-mayāgninā ।।

tāmrāyas-kānta-gandhāhvā-tārkṣā yat su-cchalaṃ rajaḥ ।
lohe bhṛṅgarajo bhṛṣṭaṃ saptāhaṃ dṛṣṭi-roga-jit ।।

-tārkṣyā yat su-cchalaṃ rajaḥ
kṛṣṇa-sarpaṃ mṛtaṃ nyasya caturaś cāpi vṛścikān ।
kṣīra-kumbhe tri-saptāhaṃ kledayitvā pramanthayet ।।

ledayitvānu manthayet ledayitvātha manthayet
tatra yan nava-nītaṃ syāt puṣṇīyāt tena kukkuṭam ।
andhas tasya puṛīṣeṇa prekṣate dhruvam añjanāt ।।

kṛṣṇa-sarpa-vasā śaṅkhaḥ katakāt phalam añjanam ।
rasa-kriyeyam a-cirād andhānāṃ darśana-pradā ।।

maricāni daśārdha-picus tāpyāt tutthāt palaṃ picur yaṣṭyāḥ ।
kṣīrārdra-dagdham añjanam a-pratisārākhyam uttamaṃ timire ।।

aricāni daśa dvi-palaṃ
akṣa-bīja-maricāmalaka-tvak-tuttha-yaṣṭimadhukair jala-piṣṭaiḥ ।
chāyayaiva guṭikāḥ pariśuṣkā nāśayanti timirāṇy a-cireṇa ।।

maricāmalaka-jalodbhava-tutthāñjana-tāpya-dhātubhiḥ krama-vṛddhaiḥ ।
ṣaṇ-mākṣika iti yogas timirārma-kleda-kāca-kaṇḍū-hantā ।।

imirārma-kleda-kāca-kaṇḍū-hā 
timirārma-kleda-kāca-kaṇḍū-ghnaḥ
ratnāni rūpyaṃ sphaṭikaṃ suvarṇaṃ sroto-'ñjanaṃ tāmram ayaḥ sa-śaṅkhaṃ ।
ku-candanaṃ lohita-gairikaṃ ca cūrṇāñjanaṃ sarva-dṛg-āmaya-ghnam ।।

tila-tailam akṣa-tailaṃ bhṛṅga-sva-raso asanāc ca niryūhaḥ ।
āyasa-pātra-vipakvaṃ karoti dṛṣṭer balaṃ nasyam ।।

aroti dṛṣṭer balaṃ nasyāt
doṣānurodhena ca naika-śas taṃ snehāsra-visrāvaṇa-reka-nasyaiḥ ।
upācared añjana-mūrdha-vasti-vasti-kriyā-tarpaṇa-lepa-sekaiḥ ।।
sāmānyaṃ sādhanam idaṃ prati-doṣam ataḥ śṛṇu ।।
vāta-je timire tatra daśa-mūlāmbhasā ghṛtam ।
kṣīre catur-guṇe śreṣṭhā-kalka-pakvaṃ pibet tataḥ ।।

tri-phalā-pañca-mūlānāṃ kaṣāyaṃ kṣīra-saṃyutam ।
eraṇḍa-taila-saṃyuktaṃ yojayec ca virecanam ।।

raṇḍa-taila-saṃmiśraṃ ojayeta virecanam
sa-mūla-jāla-jīvantī-tulāṃ droṇe ambhasaḥ pacet ।
aṣṭa-bhāga-sthite tasmiṃs taila-prasthaṃ payaḥ-same ।।

aila-prasthaṃ payaḥ-samam
balā-tritaya-jīvantī-varī-mūlaiḥ palonmitaiḥ ।
yaṣṭī-palaiś caturbhiś ca loha-pātre vipācayet ।।

alā-tri-jāta-jīvantī-
loha eva sthitaṃ māsaṃ nāvanād ūrdhva-jatru-jān ।
vāta-pittāmayān hanti tad viśeṣād dṛg-āśrayān ।।

oha-pātra-sthitaṃ māsaṃ ad viśeṣād dṛg-āmayān
keśāsya-kandharā-skandha-puṣṭi-lāvaṇya-kānti-dam ।
sitairaṇḍa-jaṭā-siṃhī-phala-dāru-vacā-nataiḥ ।।

-puṣṭi-lāvaṇya-kānti-kṛt
ghoṣayā bilva-mūlaiś ca tailaṃ pakvaṃ payo-'nvitam ।
nasyaṃ sarvordhva-jatrūttha-vāta-śleṣmāmayārti-jit ।।

śatāhvā-bilva-mūlaiś ca
vasāñjane ca vaiyāghrī vārāhī vā praśasyate ।
gṛdhrāhi-kukkuṭotthā vā madhukenānvitā pṛthak ।।

pratyañjane ca sroto-jaṃ rasa-kṣīra-ghṛte kramāt ।
niṣiktaṃ pūrva-vad yojyaṃ timira-ghnam an-uttamam ।।

asa-kṣīra-ghṛtaiḥ kramāt
na ced evaṃ śamaṃ yāti tatas tarpaṇam ācaret ।
śatāhvā-kuṣṭha-nalada-kākolī-dvaya-yaṣṭibhiḥ ।।

prapauṇḍarīka-sarala-pippalī-devadārubhiḥ ।
sarpir aṣṭa-guṇa-kṣīraṃ pakvaṃ tarpaṇam uttamam ।।

medasas tad-vad aiṇeyād dugdha-siddhāt khajāhatāt ।
uddhṛtaṃ sādhitaṃ tejo madhukośīra-candanaiḥ ।।

śvāvic-chalyaka-godhānāṃ dakṣa-tittiri-barhiṇām ।
pṛthak pṛthag anenaiva vidhinā kalpayed vasām ।।

śvāvic-chalyaka-godhānām śvā-viṣkirāka-godhānām 
ṛkṣa-tittiri-barhiṇām
prasādanaṃ snehanaṃ ca puṭa-pākaṃ prayojayet ।
vāta-pīnasa-vac cātra nirūhaṃ sānuvāsanam ।।

irūhaṃ cānuvāsanam
pitta-je timire sarpir jīvanīya-phala-trayaiḥ ।
vipācitaṃ pāyayitvā snigdhasya vyadhayet sirām ।।

śarkarailā-trivṛc-cūrṇair madhu-yuktair virecayet ।
su-śītān seka-lepādīn yuñjyān netrāsya-mūrdhasu ।।

śārivā-padmakośīra-muktā-śābara-candanaiḥ ।
vartiḥ śastāñjane cūrṇas tathā pattrotpalāñjanaiḥ ।।

artiḥ śastāñjanaṃ cūrṇas athā padmotpalāñjanaiḥ
sa-nāgapuṣpa-karpūra-yaṣṭy-āhva-svarṇa-gairikaiḥ ।
sauvīrāñjana-tutthaka-śṛṅgī-dhātrī-phala-sphaṭika-karpūram ।।

pañcāṃśaṃ pañcāṃśaṃ try-aṃśam athaikāṃśam añjanaṃ timira-ghnam ।
nasyaṃ cājyaṃ śṛtaṃ kṣīra-jīvanīya-sitotpalaiḥ ।।

śleṣmodbhave amṛtā-kvātha-varā-kaṇa-śṛtaṃ ghṛtam ।
vidhyet sirāṃ pīta-vato dadyāc cānu virecanam ।।

kvāthaṃ pūgābhayā-śuṇṭhī-kṛṣṇā-kumbha-nikumbha-jam ।
hrīvera-dāru-dvi-niśā-kṛṣṇā-kalkaiḥ payo-'nvitaiḥ ।।

dvi-pañca-mūla-niryūhe tailaṃ pakvaṃ ca nāvanam ।
śaṅkha-priyaṅgu-nepālī-kaṭu-trika-phala-trikaiḥ ।।

dṛg-vaimalyāya vi-malā vartiḥ syāt kokilā punaḥ ।
kṛṣṇa-loha-rajo-vyoṣa-saindhava-tri-phalāñjanaiḥ ।।

artiḥ syāt kaulikā punaḥ
śaśa-go-khara-siṃhoṣṭra-dvi-jā lālāṭam asthi ca ।
śveta-go-vāla-marica-śaṅkha-candana-phenakam ।।

piṣṭaṃ stanyājya-dugdhābhyāṃ vartis timira-śukra-jit ।
rakta-je pitta-vat siddhiḥ śītaiś cāsraṃ prasādayet ।।

madhūka-sārāñjana-tāmra-tri-kaṭuka-viḍaṅga-pauṇḍarīkāṇi ।
sa-lavaṇa-tuttha-tri-phalā-lodhrāṇi nabho-'mbu-piṣṭāni ।।

vartiś catur-daśāṅgī nayanāmaya-nāśanī śilā-stambhe ।
likhitā hitāya jagatas timirāpaharī viśeṣeṇa ।।

eka-guṇā māgadhikā dvi-guṇā ca harītakī salila-piṣṭā ।
vartir iyaṃ timira-paṭala-kāca-kaṇḍv-asra-harī ।।

drākṣayā nalada-lodhra-yaṣṭibhiḥ śaṅkha-tāmra-hima-padma-padmakaiḥ ।
sotpalaiś chagala-dugdha-vartitair asra-jaṃ timiram āśu naśyati ।।

rākṣayā nalada-lodhra-yaṣṭikā- -śaṅkha-tāmra-hima-padma-padmakaiḥ 
-śaṅkha-tāmra-hima-padma-pattrakaiḥ
saṃsarga-saṃnipātotthe yathā-doṣodayaṃ kriyā ।
siddhaṃ madhūka-kṛmijin-maricāmaradārubhiḥ ।।

sa-kṣīraṃ nāvanaṃ tailaṃ piṣṭair lepo mukhasya ca ।
nata-nīlotpalānantā-yaṣṭy-āhva-suniṣaṇṇakaiḥ ।।

sādhitaṃ nāvane tailaṃ śiro-vastau ca śasyate ।
dadyād uśīra-niryūhe cūrṇitaṃ kaṇa-saindhavam ।।

ādhitaṃ nāvanaṃ tailaṃ
tat srutaṃ sa-ghṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ pacet kṣaudraṃ ghane kṣipet ।
śīte cāsmin hitam idaṃ sarva-je timire añjanam ।।

ac chṛtaṃ sa-ghṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ
asthīni majja-pūrṇāni sat-tvānāṃ rātri-cāriṇām ।
sroto-jāñjana-yuktāni vahaty ambhasi vāsayet ।।

roto-'ñjanena yuktāni
māsaṃ viṃśati-rātraṃ vā tataś coddhṛtya śoṣayet ।
sa-meṣaśṛṅgī-puṣpāṇi sa-yaṣṭy-āhvāni tāny anu ।।

a-yaṣṭy-āhvāni tāni tu
cūrṇitāny añjanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ timire sāṃnipātike ।
kāce apy eṣā kriyā muktvā sirāṃ yantra-nipīḍitāḥ ।।

irā yantra-nipīḍitāḥ irāṃ yantra-nipīḍanāt
āndhyāya syur malā dadyāt srāvye tv asre jalaukasaḥ ।
guḍaḥ pheno añjanaṃ kṛṣṇā maricaṃ kuṅkumād rajaḥ ।।

āndhyāya syur ato dadyāt
rasa-kriyeyaṃ sa-kṣaudrā kāca-yāpanam añjanam ।
nakulāndhe tri-doṣotthe taimirya-vihito vidhiḥ ।।

aimirya-vidhi-vat kriyāḥ
rasa-kriyā ghṛta-kṣaudra-go-maya-sva-rasa-drutaiḥ ।
tārkṣya-gairika-tālīśair niśāndhe hitam añjanam ।।

iśāndhye hitam añjanam
dadhnā vighṛṣṭaṃ maricaṃ rātry-andhe añjanam uttamam ।
karañjikotpala-svarṇa-gairikāmbho-ja-kesaraiḥ ।।

ātry-andhāñjanam uttamam ārañjikotpala-svarṇa-
piṣṭair go-maya-toyena vartir doṣāndha-nāsinī ।
ajā-mūtreṇa vā kauntī-kṛṣṇā-sroto-ja-saindhavaiḥ ।।

artir doṣāndhya-nāsinī
kālānusārī-tri-kaṭu-tri-phalāla-manaḥśilāḥ ।
sa-phenāś chāga-dugdhena rātry-andhe vartayo hitāḥ ।।

ātry-āndhye vartayo hitāḥ
saṃniveśya yakṛn-madhye pippalīr a-dahan pacet ।
tāḥ śuṣkā madhunā ghṛṣṭā niśāndhe śreṣṭham añjanam ।।

iśāndhye śreṣṭham añjanam aktāndhye śreṣṭham añjanam
khādec ca plīha-yakṛtī māhiṣe taila-sarpiṣā ।
ghṛte siddhāni jīvantyāḥ pallavāni ca bhakṣayet ।।

tathātimuktakairaṇḍa-śephāly-abhīru-jāni ca ।
bhṛṣṭaṃ ghṛtaṃ kumbhayoneḥ pattraiḥ pāne ca pūjitam ।।

iddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ kumbha-yoneḥ attraiḥ pāne ati-pūjitam
dhūmarākhyāmla-pittoṣṇa-vidāhe jīrṇa-sarpiṣā ।
snigdhaṃ virecayec chītaiḥ śītair dihyāc ca sarvataḥ ।।

go-śakṛd-rasa-dugdhājyair vipakvaṃ śasyate añjanam ।
svarṇa-gairika-tālīśa-cūrṇāvāpā rasa-kriyā ।।

medā-śābarakānantā-mañjiṣṭhā-dārvi-yaṣṭibhiḥ ।
kṣīrāṣṭāṃśaṃ ghṛtaṃ pakvaṃ sa-tailaṃ nāvanaṃ hitam ।।

tarpaṇaṃ kṣīra-sarpiḥ syād a-śāmyati sirā-vyadhaḥ ।
cintābhighāta-bhī-śoka-raukṣyāt sotkaṭakāsanāt ।।

-rūkṣāmla-kaṭukāśanāt
vireka-nasya-vamana-puṭa-pākādi-vibhramāt ।
vidagdhāhāra-vamanāt kṣut-tṛṣṇādi-vidhāraṇāt ।।

akṣi-rogāvasānāc ca paśyet timira-rogi-vat ।
yathā-svaṃ tatra yuñjīta doṣādīn vīkṣya bheṣajam ।।

sūryoparāgānala-vidyud-ādi-vilokanenopahatekṣaṇasya ।
saṃtarpaṇaṃ snigdha-himādi kāryaṃ tathāñjanaṃ hema ghṛtena ghṛṣṭam ।।

cakṣū-rakṣāyāṃ sarva-kālaṃ manuṣyair yatnaḥ kartavyo jīvite yāvad icchā ।
vyartho loko ayaṃ tulya-rātrin-divānāṃ puṃsām andhānāṃ vidyamāne api vitte ।।

tri-phalā rudhira-srutir viśuddhir manaso nirvṛtir añjanaṃ sa-nasyam ।
śakunāśana-tā sa-pāda-pūjā ghṛta-pānaṃ ca sadaiva netra-rakṣā ।।

anaso nirvṛtir añjanaṃ ca nasyam śayanāsana-tā sa-pāda-pūjā 
śayanāsana-toṣa-pāda-pūjā
a-hitād aśanāt sadā nivṛttir bhṛśa-bhās-vac-cala-sūkṣma-vīkṣaṇāc ca ।
muninā niminopadiṣṭam etat paramaṃ rakṣaṇam īkṣaṇasya puṃsām ।।

uttarasthāna
vidhyet su-jātaṃ niṣ-prekṣyaṃ liṅga-nāśaṃ kaphodbhavam ।
āvartaky-ādibhiḥ ṣaḍbhir vivarjitam upadravaiḥ ।।

so a-saṃjāto hi viṣamo dadhi-mastu-nibhas tanuḥ ।
śalākayāvakṛṣṭo api punar ūrdhvaṃ prapadyate ।।

unar ūrdhvaṃ pravartate
karoti vedanāṃ tīvrāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ ca sthagayet punaḥ ।
śleṣmalaiḥ pūryate cāśu so anyaiḥ sopadravaś cirāt ।।

o anyaiḥ sopadravaiś cirāt
ślaiṣmiko liṅga-nāśo hi sita-tvāc chleṣmaṇaḥ sitaḥ ।
tasyānya-doṣābhibhavād bhavaty ā-nīla-tā gadaḥ ।।

havaty ā-nīla-tā gade havaty ā-nīlikā gade
tatrāvarta-calā dṛṣṭir āvartaky aruṇāsitā ।
śarkarārka-payo-leśa-niciteva ghanāti ca ।।

āvartaky aruṇā sitā
rājī-matī dṛṅ nicitā śāli-śūkābha-rājibhiḥ ।
viṣama-cchinna-dagdhābhā sa-ruk chinnāṃśukā smṛtā ।।

dṛṣṭiḥ kāṃsya-sama-cchāyā candrakī candrakākṛtiḥ ।
chattrābhā naika-varṇā ca chattrakī nāma nīlikā ।।

na vidhyed a-sirārhāṇāṃ na tṛṭ-pīnasa-kāsinām ।
nā-jīrṇi-bhīru-vamita-śiraḥ-karṇākṣi-śūlinām ।।

a dṛk-pīnasa-kāsinām
atha sādhāraṇe kāle śuddha-saṃbhojitātmanaḥ ।
deśe prakāśe pūrvāhṇe bhiṣag jānūcca-pīṭha-gaḥ ।।

yantritasyopaviṣṭasya svinnākṣasya mukhānilaiḥ ।
aṅguṣṭha-mṛdite netre dṛṣṭau dṛṣṭvotplutaṃ malam ।।

svāṃ nāsāṃ prekṣamāṇasya niṣ-kampaṃ mūrdhni dhārite ।
kṛṣṇād ardhāṅgulaṃ muktvā tathārdhārdham apāṅgataḥ ।।

va-nāsāṃ prekṣamāṇasya ad ardhārdham apāṅgataḥ
tarjanī-madhyamāṅguṣṭhaiḥ śalākāṃ niś-calaṃ dhṛtām ।
daiva-cchidraṃ nayet pārśvād ūrdhvam āmanthayan iva ।।

savyaṃ dakṣiṇa-hastena netraṃ savyena cetarat ।
vidhyet su-viddhe śabdaḥ syād a-ruk cāmbu-lava-srutiḥ ।।

sāntvayann āturaṃ cānu netraṃ stanyena secayet ।
śalākāyās tato agreṇa nirlikhen netra-maṇḍalam ।।

irlikhed dṛṣṭi-maṇḍalam
a-bādhamānaḥ śanakair nāsāṃ prati nudaṃs tataḥ ।
ucchiṅghanāc cāpahared dṛṣṭi-maṇḍala-gaṃ kapham ।।

cchiṅkhanāc cāpahared
sthire doṣe cale vāti svedayed akṣi bāhyataḥ ।
atha dṛṣṭeṣu rūpeṣu śalākām āharec chanaiḥ ।।

thire doṣe cale vāpi
ghṛtāplutaṃ picuṃ dattvā baddhākṣaṃ śāyayet tataḥ ।
viddhād anyena pārśvena tam uttānaṃ dvayor vyadhe ।।

yadhād anyena pārśvena
nivāte śayane abhyakta-śiraḥ-pādaṃ hite ratam ।
kṣavathuṃ kāsam udgāraṃ ṣṭhīvanaṃ pānam ambhasaḥ ।।

-śiro-gātraṃ hite ratam
adho-mukha-sthitiṃ snānaṃ danta-dhāvana-bhakṣaṇam ।
saptāhaṃ nācaret sneha-pīta-vac cātra yantraṇā ।।

śaktito laṅghayet seko ruji koṣṇena sarpiṣā ।
sa-vyoṣāmalakaṃ vāṭyam aśnīyāt sa-ghṛtaṃ dravam ।।

vilepīṃ vā try-ahāc cāsya kvāthair muktvākṣi secayet ।
vāta-ghnaiḥ saptame tv ahni sarva-thaivākṣi mocayet ।।

yantraṇām anurudhyeta dṛṣṭer ā-sthairya-lābhataḥ ।
rūpāṇi sūkṣma-dīptāni sahasā nāvalokayet ।।

śopha-rāga-rujādīnām adhimanthasya codbhavaḥ ।
a-hitair vedha-doṣāc ca yathā-svaṃ tān upācaret ।।

-hitair vedhya-doṣāc ca athā-svaṃ tān upakramet
kalkitāḥ sa-ghṛtā dūrvā-yava-gairika-śārivāḥ ।
mukhālepe prayoktavyā rujā-rāgopaśāntaye ।।

sa-sarṣapās tilās tad-van mātuluṅga-rasāplutāḥ ।
payasyā-śārivā-pattra-mañjiṣṭhā-madhuyaṣṭibhiḥ ।।

ajā-kṣīra-yutair lepaḥ sukhoṣṇaḥ śarma-kṛt param ।
lodhra-saindhava-mṛdvīkā-madhukaiś chāgalaṃ payaḥ ।।

jā-kṣīrānvitair lepaḥ
śṛtam āścyotanaṃ yojyaṃ rujā-rāga-vināśanam ।
madhukotpala-kuṣṭhair vā drākṣā-lākṣā-sitānvitaiḥ ।।

adhukotpala-kuṣṭhailā- rākṣā-lākṣā-rasānvitaiḥ -drākṣā-lākṣā-sitānvitaiḥ 
-drākṣā-lākṣā-rasānvitaiḥ
vāta-ghna-siddhe payasi śṛtaṃ sarpiś catur-guṇe ।
padmakādi-pratīvāpaṃ sarva-karmasu śasyate ।।

sirāṃ tathān-upaśame snigdha-svinnasya mokṣayet ।
manthoktāṃ ca kriyāṃ kuryād vedhe rūḍhe añjanaṃ mṛdu ।।

yadhe rūḍhe añjanaṃ mṛdu
āḍhakī-mūla-marica-haritāla-rasāñjanaiḥ ।
viddhe akṣṇi sa-guḍā vartir yojyā divyāmbu-peṣitā ।।

jātī-śirīṣa-dhava-meṣaviṣāṇi-puṣpa-vaiḍūrya-mauktika-phalaṃ payasā su-piṣṭam ।
ājena tāmram amunā pratanu pradigdhaṃ saptāhataḥ punar idaṃ payasaiva piṣṭam ।। 

।।

ātī-śirīṣa-dhava-meṣaviṣāṇa-puṣpa-
piṇḍāñjanaṃ hitam an-ātapa-śuṣkam akṣṇi viddhe prasāda-jananaṃ bala-kṛc ca dṛṣṭeḥ ।
sroto-ja-vidruma-śilāmbu-dhi-phena-tīkṣṇair asyaiva tulyam uditaṃ guṇa-kalpanābhiḥ ।।

।।

roto-ja-vidruma-śilārṇava-phena-tīkṣṇair

uttarasthāna
vātena netre abhiṣyaṇṇe nāsānāho alpa-śopha-tā ।
śaṅkhākṣi-bhrū-lalāṭasya toda-sphuraṇa-bhedanam ।।

ātena netre abhiṣyande śaṅkhākṣi-bhrū-lalāṭāsya- 
-toda-sphuraṇa-bhedanam
śuṣkālpā dūṣikā śītam acchaṃ cāśru calā rujaḥ ।
nimeṣonmeṣaṇaṃ kṛcchrāj jantūnām iva sarpaṇam ।।

ccham aśru calā rujaḥ
akṣy ādhmātam ivābhāti sūkṣmaiḥ śalyair ivācitam ।
snigdhoṣṇaiś copaśamanaṃ so abhiṣyanda upekṣitaḥ ।।

nigdhoṣṇecchopaśamanaṃ
adhimantho bhavet tatra karṇayor nadanaṃ bhramaḥ ।
araṇyeva ca mathyante lalāṭākṣi-bhruvādayaḥ ।।

hatādhimanthaḥ so api syāt pramādāt tena vedanāḥ ।
aneka-rūpā jāyante vraṇo dṛṣṭau ca dṛṣṭi-hā ।।

manyākṣi-śaṅkhato vāyur anyato vā pravartayan ।
vyathāṃ tīvrām a-paicchilya-rāga-śophaṃ vilocanam ।।

nyato vā pravartayet
saṃkocayati pary-aśru so anyato-vāta-saṃjñitaḥ ।
tad-vaj jihmaṃ bhaven netram ūnaṃ vā vāta-paryaye ।।

ad-vaj jihmaṃ bhaven netraṃ ad-van netraṃ bhavej jihmam 
śūnaṃ vā vāta-paryaye
dāho dhūmāyanaṃ śophaḥ śyāva-tā vartmano bahiḥ ।
antaḥ-kledo aśru pītoṣṇaṃ rāgaḥ pītābha-darśanam ।।

kṣārokṣita-kṣatākṣi-tvaṃ pittābhiṣyanda-lakṣaṇam ।
jvalad-aṅgāra-kīrṇābhaṃ yakṛt-piṇḍa-sama-prabham ।।

adhimanthe bhaven netraṃ syande tu kapha-saṃbhave ।
jāḍyaṃ śopho mahān kaṇḍūr nidrānnān-abhinandanam ।।

sāndra-snigdha-bahu-śveta-picchā-vad-dūṣikāśru-tā ।
adhimanthe nataṃ kṛṣṇam unnataṃ śukla-maṇḍalam ।।

-picchā-vad-dūṣikāsra-tā
praseko nāsikādhmānaṃ pāṃsu-pūrṇam ivekṣaṇam ।
raktāśru-rājī-dūṣīkā-rakta-maṇḍala-darśanam ।।

aktāsra-rājī-dūṣīkā- -śukla-maṇḍala-darśanam
rakta-syandena nayanaṃ sa-pitta-syanda-lakṣaṇam ।
manthe akṣi tāmra-pary-antam utpāṭana-samāna-ruk ।।

rāgeṇa bandhūka-nibhaṃ tāmyati sparśanā-kṣamam ।
asṛṅ-nimagnāriṣṭābhaṃ kṛṣṇam agny-ābha-darśanam ।।

adhimanthā yathā-svaṃ ca sarve syandādhika-vyathāḥ ।
śaṅkha-danta-kapoleṣu kapāle cāti-ruk-karāḥ ।।

vāta-pittāturaṃ gharṣa-toda-bhedopadeha-vat ।
rūkṣa-dāruṇa-vartmākṣi kṛcchronmīla-nimīlanam ।।

āta-pittottaraṃ gharṣa-
vikūṇana-viśuṣka-tva-śītecchā-śūla-pāka-vat ।
uktaḥ śuṣkādi-pāko yaṃ sa-śophaḥ syāt tribhir malaiḥ ।।

ikūṇanaṃ viśuṣkaṃ ca ikūṇena viśuṣka-tvaṃ 
śītecchā-śūla-pāka-vat
sa-raktais tatra śopho ati-rug-dāha-ṣṭhīvanādi-mān ।
pakvodumbara-saṃkāśaṃ jāyate śukla-maṇḍalam ।।

aśrūṣṇa-śīta-viśada-picchilāccha-ghanaṃ muhuḥ ।
alpa-śophe alpa-śophas tu pāko anyair lakṣaṇais tathā ।।

lpa-śopho alpa-śophas tu
akṣi-pākātyaye śophaḥ saṃrambhaḥ kaluṣāśru-tā ।
kaphopadigdham asitaṃ sitaṃ prakleda-rāga-vat ।।

aphena digdham asitaṃ
dāho darśana-saṃrodho vedanāś cān-avasthitāḥ ।
anna-sāro amla-tāṃ nītaḥ pitta-raktolbaṇair malaiḥ ।।

sirābhir netram ārūḍhaḥ karoti śyāva-lohitam ।
sa-śopha-dāha-pākāśru bhṛśaṃ cāvila-darśanam ।।

amloṣito ayam ity uktā gadāḥ ṣo-ḍaśa sarva-gāḥ ।
hatādhimantham eteṣu sākṣi-pākātyayaṃ tyajet ।।

atādhimanthaṃ caiteṣu
vātodbhūtaḥ pañca-rātreṇa dṛṣṭiṃ saptāhena śleṣma-jāto adhimanthaḥ ।
raktotpanno hanti tad-vat tri-rātrān mithyācārāt paittikaḥ sadya eva ।।

aptāhena śleṣma-jaś cādhimanthaḥ

uttarasthāna
prāg-rūpa eva syandeṣu tīkṣṇaṃ gaṇḍūṣa-nāvanam ।
kārayed upavāsaṃ ca kopād anya-tra vāta-jāt ।।

dāhopadeha-rāgāśru-śopha-śāntyai biḍālakam ।
kuryāt sarva-tra pattrailā-marica-svarṇa-gairikaiḥ ।।

sa-rasāñjana-yaṣṭy-āhva-nata-candana-saindhavaiḥ ।
saindhavaṃ nāgaraṃ tārkṣyaṃ bhṛṣṭaṃ maṇḍena sarpiṣaḥ ।।

hṛṣṭaṃ maṇḍena sarpiṣaḥ
badarī-pattra-yaṣṭy-āhva-pathyāmalaka-tutthakam ।
antar-dhūmaṃ dahet sadyaḥ kope tac-cūrṇaṃ vāta-je ।।

vāta-je ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaṃ vā yojyaṃ śabara-deśa-jam ।
māṃsī-padmaka-kālīya-yaṣṭy-āhvaiḥ pitta-raktayoḥ ।।

ojyaṃ śābara-deśa-jam āṃsī-padmaka-kākolī- manohvā-phalinī-kṣaudraiḥ kaphe sarvais tu sarva-je ।।
sita-marica-bhāgam ekaṃ catur-manohvaṃ dvir aṣṭa-śābarakam ।।saṃcūrṇya vastra-baddhaṃ prakupita-mātre avaguṇṭhanaṃ netre ।।
aṃcūrṇyam ati-prabaddhaṃ rakupita-mātre avaguṇṭhanam idaṃ
netre
dhātu-śuṇṭhy-abhayā-tārkṣyaṃ bahir-lepo akṣi-roga-hā ।।

hātu-śuṇṭhy-abhayā-tārkṣya- -bahir-lepo 
akṣi-roga-hā
harītakī-saindhava-tārkṣya-śīlaiḥ sa-gairikaiḥ sva-sva-kara-pramṛṣṭaiḥ ।
bahiḥ-pralepaṃ nayanasya kuryāt sarvākṣi-roga-praśamārtham etat ।।

āraṇyāś chagaṇa-rase paṭāvabaddhāḥ su-svinnā nakha-vi-tuṣī-kṛtāḥ kulatthāḥ ।
tac-cūrṇaṃ sakṛd avacūrṇanān niśīthe netrāṇāṃ vidhamati sadya eva kopam ।।

āraṇyāś chagaṇa-rase paṭāvanaddhāḥ
ghoṣābhayā-tutthaka-yaṣṭi-lodhrair mūtī su-sūkṣmaiḥ ślatha-vastra-baddhaiḥ ।
tāmra-stha-dhānyāmla-nimagna-mūrtir artiṃ jayaty akṣiṇi naika-rūpām ।।

hoṣābhayā-tutthaka-yaṣṭi-lodhraiḥ yoṣābhayā-tutthaka-yaṣṭi-lodhrair uṇḍī su-sūkṣmaiḥ ślatha-vastra-baddhaiḥ iṣṭaiḥ su-sūkṣmaiḥ ślatha-vastra-baddhaiḥ 
āmrāccha-dhānyāmla-nimagna-mūrtir
ṣo-ḍaśabhiḥ salila-palaiḥ palaṃ tathaikaṃ kaṭaṅkaṭeryāḥ siddham ।
seko aṣṭa-bhāga-śiṣṭaḥ kṣaudra-yutaḥ sarva-doṣa-kupite netre ।।

ṣaudra-yutaḥ sarva-doṣa-prakupite netre
vāta-pitta-kapha-saṃnipāta-jāṃ netrayor bahu-vidhām api vyathām ।
śīghram eva jayati prayojitaḥ śigru-pallava-rasaḥ sa-mākṣikaḥ ।।

taruṇam urubūka-pattraṃ mūlaṃ ca vibhidya siddham āje kṣīre ।
vātābhiṣyanda-rujaṃ sadyo vinihanti saktu-piṇḍikā coṣṇā ।।

ūlaṃ ca vicūrṇya siddham āje kṣīre
āścyotanaṃ māruta-je kvātho bilvādibhir hitaḥ ।
koṣṇaḥ sahairaṇḍa-jaṭā-bṛhatī-madhu-śigrubhiḥ ।।

hrīvera-vakra-śārṅgaṣṭodumbara-tvakṣu sādhitam ।
sāmbhasā payasājena śūlāścyotanam uttamam ।।

ṃdumbara-tvak-prasādhitam ṃdumbara-plakṣa-sādhitam
lodhrāmalaka-rasāñja[na]-bimbitikā-pattra-tubarikā-tutthaiḥ ।
āścyotanam idam akṣṇoḥ prasahya sadyaḥ prakopa-haram ।।

mañjiṣṭhā-rajanī-lākṣā-drākṣarddhi-madhukotpalaiḥ ।
kvāthaḥ sa-śarkaraḥ śītaḥ secanaṃ rakta-pitta-jit ।।

-drākṣā-dvi-madhukotpalaiḥ
kaseru-yaṣṭy-āhva-rajas tāntave śithilaṃ sthitam ।
apsu divyāsu nihitaṃ hitaṃ syande asra-pitta-je ।।

āntave śithile sthitam
puṇḍra-yaṣṭī-niśā-mūtī plutā stanye sa-śarkare ।
chāga-dugdhe atha-vā dāha-rug-rāgāśru-nivartanī ।।

śveta-lodhraṃ sa-madhukaṃ ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaṃ su-cūrṇitam ।
vastra-sthaṃ stanya-mṛditaṃ pitta-raktābhighāta-jit ।।

nāgara-tri-phalā-nimba-vāsā-lodhra-rasaḥ kaphe ।
koṣṇam āścyotanaṃ miśrair bheṣajaiḥ sāṃnipātike ।।

-vāsā-lodhra-rasāḥ kaphe -vāsā-lodhra-rasaṃ kaphe
sarpiḥ purāṇaṃ pavane pitte śarkarayānvitam ।
vyoṣa-siddhaṃ kaphe pītvā yava-kṣārāvacūrṇitam ।।

itte śarkarayā yutam
srāvayed rudhiraṃ bhūyas tataḥ snigdhaṃ virecayet ।
ānūpa-vesavāreṇa śiro-vadana-lepanam ।।

uṣṇena śūle dāhe tu payaḥ-sarpir-yutair himaiḥ ।
timira-pratiṣedhaṃ ca vīkṣya yuñjyād yathā-yatham ।।

ayam eva vidhiḥ sarvo manthādiṣv api śasyate ।
a-śāntau sarva-thā manthe bhruvor upari dāhayet ।।

rūpyaṃ rūkṣeṇa go-dadhnā limpen nīla-tvam āgate ।
śuṣke tu mastunā vartir vātākṣy-āmaya-nāśinī ।।

iptaṃ nīla-tvam āgate ipte nīla-tvam āgate
sumanaḥ-korakāḥ śaṅkhas tri-phalā madhukaṃ balā ।
pitta-raktāpahā vartiḥ piṣṭā divyena vāriṇā ।।

umanaḥ-kṣārakāḥ śaṅkhas
saindhavaṃ tri-phalā vyoṣaṃ śaṅkhanābhiḥ samudra-jaḥ ।
phena aileyakaṃ sarjo vartiḥ śleṣmākṣi-roga-nut ।।

prapauṇḍarīkaṃ yaṣṭy-āhvaṃ dārvī cāṣṭa-palaṃ pacet ।
jala-droṇe rase pūte punaḥ pakve ghane kṣipet ।।

puṣpāñjanād daśa-palaṃ karṣaṃ ca maricāt tataḥ ।
kṛtaś cūrṇo atha-vā vartiḥ sarvābhiṣyanda-saṃbhavān ।।

hanti rāga-rujā-gharṣān sadyo dṛṣṭiṃ prasādayet ।
ayaṃ pāśupato yogo rahasyaṃ bhiṣajāṃ param ।।

śuṣkākṣi-pāke haviṣaḥ pānam akṣṇoś ca tarpaṇam ।
ghṛtena jīvanīyena nasyaṃ tailena vāṇunā ।।

asyaṃ tailena cāṇunā
pariṣeko hitaś cātra payaḥ koṣṇaṃ sa-saindhavam ।
sarpir-yuktaṃ stanya-piṣṭam añjanaṃ ca mahauṣadham ।।

arpir-yuktaṃ stanya-ghṛṣṭam
vasā vānūpa-sat-tvotthā kiñ-cit-saindhava-nāgarā ।
ghṛtāktān darpaṇe ghṛṣṭān keśān mallaka-saṃpuṭe ।।

asā cānūpa-sat-tvotthā
dagdhvājya-piṣṭā loha-sthā sā maṣī śreṣṭham añjanam ।
sa-śophe vālpa-śophe ca snigdhasya vyadhayet sirām ।।

a-śophe cālpa-śophe ca
rekaḥ snigdhe punar drākṣā-pathyā-kvātha-trivṛd-ghṛtaiḥ ।
śveta-lodhraṃ ghṛte bhṛṣṭaṃ cūrṇitaṃ tāntava-sthitam ।।

śveta-lodhraṃ ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaṃ
uṣṇāmbunā vimṛditaṃ sekaḥ śūla-haraḥ param ।
dārvī-prapauṇḍarīkasya kvātho vāścyotane hitaḥ ।।

ārvyāḥ prapauṇḍarīkasya yaṣṭī-himotpala-kṣīraiḥ kuryān mūrdhasya lepanam ।।
saṃdhāvāṃś ca prayuñjīta gharṣa-rāgāśru-rug-gharān ।।
tāmraṃ lohe mūtra-ghṛṣṭaṃ prayuktaṃ netre sarpir-dhūpitaṃ vedanā-ghnam ।
tāmre ghṛṣṭo gavya-dadhnaḥ saro vā yuktaḥ kṛṣṇā-saindhavābhyāṃ variṣṭhaḥ ।।

śaṅkhaṃ tāmre stanya-ghṛṣṭaṃ ghṛtāktaiḥ śamyāḥ pattrair dhūpitaṃ tad yavaiś ca ।
netre yuktaṃ hanti saṃdhāva-saṃjñaṃ kṣipraṃ gharṣaṃ vedanāṃ cāti-tīvrām ।।
udumbara-phalaṃ lohe ghṛṣṭaṃ stanyena dhūpitam ।।
sājyaiḥ śamī-cchadair dāha-śūla-rāgāśru-harṣa-jit ।
śigru-pallava-niryāsaḥ su-ghṛṣṭas tāmra-saṃpuṭe ।।

śigru-pallava-niryāso hṛṣṭas tāmrasya saṃpuṭe
dvi-niśā-tri-phalā-mustaiḥ pramadā-dugdha-peṣitaiḥ ।
sekaḥ sa-śarkarā-kṣaudrair abhighāta-rujāpahaḥ ।।

ramadā-dugdha-kalkitaiḥ
niṣiktaṃ tutthakaṃ vārān go-jale pañca-viṃśatim ।
stanye vā chāga-dugdhe vā sadyaḥ-kope tad añjanam ।।

ghṛtena dhūpito hanti śopha-gharṣāśru-vedanāḥ ।
tilāmbhasā mṛt-kapālaṃ kāṃsye ghṛṣṭaṃ su-dhūpitam ।।

nimba-pattrair ghṛtābhyaktair gharṣa-śūlāśru-rāga-jit ।
saṃdhāvenāñjite netre vigatauṣadha-vedane ।।

stanyenāścyotanaṃ kāryaṃ triḥ paraṃ nāñjayec ca taiḥ ।
tālīśa-pattra-capalā-nata-loha-rajo-'ñjanaiḥ ।।

-nata-loha-rasāñjanaiḥ
jātī-mukula-kāsīsa-saindhavair mūtra-peṣitaiḥ ।
tāmram ālipya saptāhaṃ dhārayet peṣayet tataḥ ।।

mūtreṇaivānu guṭikāḥ kāryāś chāyā-viśoṣitāḥ ।
tāḥ stanya-ghṛṣṭā gharṣāśru-śopha-kaṇḍū-vināśanāḥ ।।

ūtreṇa cānu guṭikāḥ uryāc chāyā-viśoṣitāḥ
vyāghrī-tvaṅ-madhukaṃ tāmra-rajo ajā-kṣīra-kalkitam ।
śamy-āmalaka-pattrājya-dhūpitaṃ śopha-ruk-praṇut ।।

-rajo ajā-kṣīra-peṣitam
amloṣite prayuñjīta pittābhiṣyanda-sādhanam ।
utkliṣṭāḥ kapha-pittāsra-nicayotthāḥ kukūṇakaḥ ।।

pakṣmoparodhaṃ śuṣkākṣi-pākaḥ pūyālaso bisaḥ ।
pothaky-amloṣito alpākhyaḥ syanda-manthā vinānilāt ।।

ete aṣṭā-daśa pillākhyā dīrgha-kālānubandhinaḥ ।
cikitsā pṛthag eteṣāṃ svaṃ svam uktātha vakṣyate ।।

vaṃ svam uktātha kathyate
pillī-bhūteṣu sāmānyād atha pillākhya-rogiṇaḥ ।
snigdhasya chardita-vataḥ sirā-vyadha-hṛtāsṛjaḥ ।।

tha pillākṣi-rogiṇaḥ
viriktasya ca vartmānu nirlikhed ā-viśuddhitaḥ ।
tutthakasya palaṃ śveta-maricāni ca viṃśatiḥ ।।

iriktasya tu vartmānu ilikhed ā-viśuddhitaḥ
triṃśatā kāñjika-palaiḥ piṣṭvā tāmre nidhāpayet ।
pillān a-pillān kurute bahu-varṣotthitān api ।।

tat sekenopadehāśru-kaṇḍū-śophāṃś ca nāśayet ।
karañja-bījaṃ surasaṃ sumanaḥ-korakāṇi ca ।।

umanaḥ-kṣārakāṇi ca
saṃkṣudya sādhayet kvāthe pūte tatra rasa-kriyā ।
añjanaṃ pilla-bhaiṣajyaṃ pakṣmaṇāṃ ca prarohaṇam ।।

rasāñjanaṃ sarja-raso rīti-puṣpaṃ manaḥśilā ।
samudra-pheno lavaṇaṃ gairikaṃ maricāni ca ।।

ātī-puṣpaṃ manaḥśilā amudra-phenaṃ lavaṇaṃ
añjanaṃ madhunā piṣṭaṃ kleda-kaṇḍū-ghnam uttamam ।
abhayā-rasa-piṣṭaṃ vā tagaraṃ pilla-nāśanam ।।

bhāvitaṃ basta-mūtreṇa sa-snehaṃ devadāru ca ।
saindhava-tri-phalā-kṛṣṇā-kaṭukā-śaṅkhanābhayaḥ ।।

a-snehaṃ devadāru vā
sa-tāmra-rajaso vartiḥ pilla-śukraka-nāśinī ।
puṣpa-kāsīsa-cūrṇo vā surasā-rasa-bhāvitaḥ ।।
tāmre daśāhaṃ tat paillya-pakṣma-śāta-jid añjanam ।।
alaṃ ca sauvīrakam añjanaṃ ca tābhyāṃ samaṃ tāmra-rajaḥ su-sūkṣmam ।
pilleṣu romāṇi niṣevito asau cūrṇaḥ karoty eka-śalākayāpi ।।

ābhyāṃ samaṃ tāmra-rajaś ca sūkṣmam illeṣu romāṇi 
niṣevito ayaṃ
lākṣā-nirguṇḍī-bhṛṅga-dārvī-rasena śreṣṭhaṃ kārpāsaṃ bhāvitaṃ sapta-kṛtvaḥ ।
dīpaḥ prajvālyaḥ sarpiṣā tat-samutthā śreṣṭhā pillānāṃ ropaṇārthe maṣī sā ।।
