śreṣṭhā pillānāṃ ropaṇārthaṃ maṣī sā vartmāvalekhaṃ bahu-śas tad-vac choṇita-mokṣaṇam ।।

punaḥ punar virekaṃ ca nityam āścyotanāñjanam ।
nāvanaṃ dhūma-pānaṃ ca pilla-rogāturo bhajet ।।

pūyālase tv a-śānte ante dāhaḥ sūkṣma-śalākayā ।
catur-ṇavatir ity akṣṇo hetu-lakṣaṇa-sādhanaiḥ ।।

ūyālase tv a-śānte tu atur-ṇavatir ity akṣṇor
paras-param a-saṃkīrṇāḥ kārtsnyena gaditā gadāḥ ।
sarva-dā ca niṣeveta svastho api nayana-priyaḥ ।।

purāṇa-yava-godhūma-śāli-ṣaṣṭika-kodravān ।
mudgādīn kapha-pitta-ghnān bhūri-sarpiḥ-pariplutān ।।

śākaṃ caivaṃ-vidhaṃ māṃsaṃ jāṅgalaṃ dāḍimaṃ sitām ।
saindhavaṃ tri-phalāṃ drākṣāṃ vāri pāne ca nābhasam ।।

ātapa-traṃ pada-trāṇaṃ vidhi-vad doṣa-śodhanam ।
varjayed vega-saṃrodham a-jīrṇādhyaśanāni ca ।।

-jīrṇādhyaśanādi ca
krodha-śoka-divā-svapna-rātri-jāgaraṇātapān ।
vidāhi viṣṭambha-karaṃ yac cehāhāra-bheṣajam ।।

-niśā-jāgaraṇāni ca idāha-viṣṭambha-karaṃ ad yad āhāra-bheṣajam 
ihārāhāra-bheṣajam
dve pāda-madhye pṛthu-saṃniveśe sire gate te bahu-dhā ca netre ।
tā mrakṣaṇodvartana-lepanādīn pāda-prayuktān nayane nayanti ।।

ve pāda-madhye pṛthu-saṃniviṣṭe āda-prayuktān nayanaṃ 
nayanti
malauṣṇya-saṃghaṭṭana-pīḍanādyais tā dūṣayante nayanāni duṣṭāḥ ।
bhajet sadā dṛṣṭi-hitāni tasmād upānad-abhyañjana-dhāvanāni ।।

aloṣṇa-saṃghaṭṭana-pīḍanādyais ṛl-loṣṭa-saṃghaṭṭana-pīḍanādyais

uttarasthāna
pratiśyāya-jala-krīḍā-karṇa-kaṇḍūyanair marut ।
mithyā-yogena śabdasya kupito anyaiś ca kopanaiḥ ।।

prāpya śrotra-sirāḥ kuryāc chūlaṃ srotasi vega-vat ।
ardhāvabhedakaṃ stambhaṃ śiśirān-abhinandanam ।।

cirāc ca pākaṃ pakvaṃ tu lasīkām alpa-śaḥ sravet ।
śrotraṃ śūnyam a-kasmāc ca syāt saṃcāra-vicāra-vat ।।

śūlaṃ pittāt sa-dāhoṣā-śītecchā-śvayathu-jvaram ।
āśu-pākaṃ prapakvaṃ ca sa-pīta-lasikā-sruti ।।

-śītecchā-śvayathur jvaraḥ
sā lasīkā spṛśed yad yat tat tat pākam upaiti ca ।
kaphāc chiro-hanu-grīvā-gauravaṃ manda-tā rujaḥ ।।

kaṇḍūḥ śvayathur uṣṇecchā pākāc chveta-ghana-srutiḥ ।
karoti śravaṇe śūlam abhighātādi-dūṣitam ।।

ākāc chveta-ghanā srutiḥ
raktaṃ pitta-samānārti kiñ-cid vādhika-lakṣaṇam ।
śūlaṃ samuditair doṣaiḥ sa-śopha-jvara-tīvra-ruk ।।

paryāyād uṣṇa-śītecchāṃ jāyate śruti-jāḍya-vat ।
pakvaṃ sitāsitā-rakta-ghana-pūya-pravāhi ca ।।

śabda-vāhi-sirā-saṃsthe śṛṇoti pavane muhuḥ ।
nādān a-kasmād vividhān karṇa-nādaṃ vadanti tam ।।

śleṣmaṇānugato vāyur nādo vā samupekṣitaḥ ।
uccaiḥ kṛcchrāc chrutiṃ kuryād badhira-tvaṃ krameṇa ca ।।

adhira-tvaṃ krameṇa vā
vātena śoṣitaḥ śleṣmā śroto limpet tato bhavet ।
rug-gauravaṃ pidhānaṃ ca sa pratīnāha-saṃjñitaḥ ।।

kaṇḍū-śophau kaphāc chrotre sthirau tat-saṃjñayā smṛtau ।
kapho vidagdhaḥ pittena sa-rujaṃ nī-rujaṃ tv api ।।

thirau tat-saṃjñitau smṛtau a-rujaṃ nī-rujaṃ tv atha
ghana-pūti-bahu-kledaṃ kurute pūti-karṇakam ।
vātādi-dūṣitaṃ śrotraṃ māṃsāsṛk-kleda-jā rujam ।।

āṃsāsṛk-kleda-jāṃ rujam
khādanto jantavaḥ kuryus tīvrāṃ sa kṛmi-karṇakaḥ ।
śrotra-kaṇḍūyanāj jāte kṣate syāt pūrva-lakṣaṇaḥ ।।

śrotaḥ-kaṇḍūyanāj jāte
vidradhiḥ pūrva-vac cānyaḥ śopho arśo arbudam īritam ।
teṣu ruk pūti-karṇa-tvaṃ badhira-tvaṃ ca bādhate ।।

ṣo-ḍhārśo arbudam īritam adhira-tvaṃ ca jāyate
garbhe anilāt saṃkucitā śaṣkulī kuci-karṇakaḥ ।
eko nī-rug aneko vā garbhe māṃsāṅkuraḥ sthiraḥ ।।

śaṣkulī kuñci-karṇakaḥ śaṣkulī kūci-karṇakaḥ 
garbhe māṃsāṅkuraḥ sthitaḥ
pippalī pippalī-mānaḥ saṃnipātād vidārikā ।
sa-varṇaḥ sa-rujaḥ stabdhaḥ śvayathuḥ sa upekṣitaḥ ।।

kaṭu-taila-nibhaṃ pakvaḥ sravet kṛcchreṇa rohati ।
saṃkocayati rūḍhā ca sā dhruvaṃ karṇa-śaṣkulīm ।।

ravan kṛcchreṇa rohati
sirā-sthaḥ kurute vāyuḥ pālī-śoṣaṃ tad-āhvayam ।
kṛśā dṛḍhā ca tantrī-vat pālī vātena tantrikā ।।

su-kumāre cirotsargāt sahasaiva pravardhite ।
karṇe śophaḥ sa-ruk pālyām aruṇaḥ paripoṭa-vān ।।

paripoṭaḥ sa pavanād utpātaḥ pitta-śoṇitāt ।
gurv-ābharaṇa-bhārādyaiḥ śyāvo rug-dāha-pāka-vān ।।

śvayathuḥ sphoṭa-piṭikā-rāgoṣā-kleda-saṃyutaḥ ।
pālyāṃ śopho anila-kaphāt sarvato nir-vyathaḥ sthiraḥ ।।

stabdhaḥ sa-varṇaḥ kaṇḍū-mān unmantho galliraś ca saḥ ।
dur-viddhe vardhite karṇe sa-kaṇḍū-dāha-pāka-ruk ।।

nmantho gallikaś ca saḥ
śvayathuḥ saṃnipātotthaḥ sa nāmnā duḥkha-vardhanaḥ ।
kaphāsṛk-kṛmi-jāḥ sūkṣmāḥ sa-kaṇḍū-kleda-vedanāḥ ।।

lihyuḥ pālīm upekṣitāḥ lehyākhyāḥ piṭikās tā hi ।
pippalī sarva-jaṃ śūlaṃ vidārī kuci-karṇakaḥ ।।

ihyākhyāḥ piṭikās tā hi idārī kūci-karṇakaḥ
eṣām a-sādhyā yāpyaikā tantrikānyāṃs tu sādhayet ।
pañca-viṃśatir ity uktāḥ karṇa-rogā vibhāgataḥ ।।

uttarasthāna
karṇa-śūle pavana-je pibed rātrau rasāśitaḥ ।
vāta-ghna-sādhitaṃ sarpiḥ karṇaṃ svinnaṃ ca pūrayet ।।

pattrāṇāṃ pṛthag aśvattha-bilvārkairaṇḍa-janmanām ।
taila-sindhūttha-digdhānāṃ svinnānāṃ puṭa-pākataḥ ।।

rasaiḥ kavoṣṇais tad-vac ca mūlakasyāralor api ।
gaṇe vāta-hare amleṣu mūtreṣu ca vipācitaḥ ।।

mahā-sneho drutaṃ hanti su-tīvrām api vedanām ।
mahataḥ pañca-mūlasya kāṣṭhāt kṣaumeṇa veṣṭitāt ।।

taila-siktāt pradīptāgrāt snehaḥ sadyo rujāpahaḥ ।
yojyaś caivaṃ bhadrakāṣṭhāt kuṣṭhāt kāṣṭhāc ca sāralāt ।।

nehaḥ sadyo rujā-haraḥ
vāta-vyādhi-pratiśyāya-vihitaṃ hitam atra ca ।
varjayec chirasā snānaṃ śītāmbhaḥ-pānam ahny api ।।

arjayec chirasaḥ snānaṃ
pitta-śūle sitā-yukta-ghṛta-snigdhaṃ virecayet ।
drākṣā-yaṣṭī-śṛtaṃ stanyaṃ śasyate karṇa-pūraṇam ।।

yaṣṭy-anantā-himośīra-kākolī-lodhra-jīvakaiḥ ।
mṛṇāla-bisa-mañjiṣṭhā-śārivābhiś ca sādhayet ।।

yaṣṭīmadhu-rasa-prastha-kṣīra-dvi-prastha-saṃyutam ।
tailasya kuḍavaṃ nasya-pūraṇābhyañjanair idam ।।

nihanti śūla-dāhoṣāḥ kevalaṃ kṣaudram eva vā ।
yaṣṭy-ādibhiś ca sa-ghṛtaiḥ karṇau dihyāt samantataḥ ।।

vāmayet pippalī-siddha-sarpiḥ-snigdhaṃ kaphodbhave ।
dhūma-nāvana-gaṇḍūṣa-svedān kuryāt kaphāpahān ।।

laśunārdraka-śigrūṇāṃ muraṅgyā mūlakasya ca ।
kadalyāḥ sva-rasaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kad-uṣṇaḥ karṇa-pūraṇe ।।

uraṅgyā mūlakasya ca hṛṅgasya mūlakasya ca
arkāṅkurān amla-piṣṭāṃs tailāktāō̃ lavaṇānvitān ।
saṃnidhāya snuhī-kāṇḍe korite tac-chadāvṛtān ।।

orite tac chadāvṛte
svedayet puṭa-pākena sa rasaḥ śūla-jit param ।
rasena bījapūrasya kapitthasya ca pūrayet ।।

śuktena pūrayitvā vā phenenānv avacūrṇayet ।
ajāvi-mūtra-vaṃśa-tvak-siddhaṃ tailaṃ ca pūraṇam ।।

-siddha-tailena pūrayet
siddhaṃ vā sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ hiṅgu-tumburu-nāgaraiḥ ।
rakta-je pitta-vat kāryaṃ sirāṃ cāśu vimokṣayet ।।

pakve pūya-vahe karṇe dhūma-gaṇḍūṣa-nāvanam ।
yuñjyān nāḍī-vidhānaṃ ca duṣṭa-vraṇa-haraṃ ca yat ।।

srotaḥ pramṛjya digdhaṃ tu dvau kālau picu-vartibhiḥ ।
pureṇa dhūpayitvā tu mākṣikeṇa prapūrayet ।।

surasādi-gaṇa-kvātha-phāṇitāktāṃ ca yojayet ।
picu-vartiṃ su-sūkṣmaiś ca tac-cūrṇair avacūrṇayet ।।

-phāṇitāktāṃ ca śīlayet -phāṇitāktāṃ prayojayet 
-phāṇitāktāṃ niyojayet
śūla-kleda-guru-tvānāṃ vidhir eṣa nivartakaḥ ।
priyaṅgu-madhukāmbaṣṭhā-dhātaky-utpala-parṇibhiḥ ।।

mañjiṣṭhā-lodhra-lākṣābhiḥ kapitthasya rasena ca ।
pacet tailaṃ tad āsrāvaṃ nigṛhṇāty āśu pūraṇāt ।।

nāda-bādhiryayoḥ kuryād vāta-śūloktam auṣadham ।
śleṣmānubandhe śleṣmāṇam prāg jayed vamanādibhiḥ ।।

eraṇḍa-śigru-varuṇa-mūlakāt pattra-je rase ।
catur-guṇe pacet tailaṃ kṣīre cāṣṭa-guṇonmite ।।

raṇḍa-śigru-taruṇa-
yaṣṭy-āhvā-kṣīra-kākolī-kalka-yuktaṃ nihanti tat ।
nāda-bādhirya-śūlāni nāvanābhyaṅga-pūraṇaiḥ ।।

-kalka-yuktaṃ hinasti tat
pakvaṃ prativiṣā-hiṅgu-miśi-tvak-svarjikoṣaṇaiḥ ।
sa-śuktaiḥ pūraṇāt tailaṃ ruk-srāvā-śruti-nāda-nut ।।

uk-srāva-śruti-nāda-nut
karṇa-nāde hitaṃ tailaṃ sarṣapotthaṃ ca pūraṇe ।
śuṣka-mūlaka-khaṇḍānāṃ kṣāro hiṅgu mahauṣadham ।।

śatapuṣpā-vacā-kuṣṭha-dāru-śigru-rasāñjanam ।
sauvarcala-yava-kṣāra-svarjikaudbhida-saindhavam ।।

bhūrja-granthi-viḍaṃ mustā madhu-śuktaṃ catur-guṇam ।
mātuluṅga-rasas tad-vat kadalī-sva-rasaś ca taiḥ ।।

pakvaṃ tailaṃ jayaty āśu su-kṛcchrān api pūraṇāt ।
kaṇḍūṃ kledaṃ ca bādhirya-pūti-karṇa-tva-ruk-kṛmīn ।।

aṇḍū-kṣveḍana-bādhirya- aṇḍū-jvalana-bādhirya-
kṣāra-tailam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mukha-dantāmayeṣu ca ।
atha suptāv iva syātāṃ karṇau raktaṃ haret tataḥ ।।

arṇau raktaṃ haret tayoḥ
sa-śopha-kledayor manda-śruter vamanam ācaret ।
bādhiryaṃ varjayed bāla-vṛddhayoś cira-jaṃ ca yat ।।

pratīnāhe parikledya sneha-svedair viśodhayet ।
karṇa-śodhanakenānu karṇaṃ tailasya pūrayet ।।

arṇaṃ tailena pūrayet
sa-śukta-saindhava-madhor mātuluṅga-rasasya vā ।
śodhanād rūkṣa-totpattau ghṛta-maṇḍasya pūraṇam ।।

a-śukta-saindhavenāśu ātuluṅga-rasena vā 
ghṛta-maṇḍena pūraṇam
kramo ayaṃ mala-pūrṇe api karṇe kaṇḍvāṃ kaphāpaham ।
nasyādi tad-vac chophe api kaṭūṣṇaiś cātra lepanam ।।

aṭūṣṇaiś cānu lepanam
karṇa-srāvoditaṃ kuryāt pūti-kṛmiṇa-karṇayoḥ ।
pūraṇaṃ kaṭu-tailena viśeṣāt kṛmi-karṇake ।।

ūti-kṛmila-karṇayoḥ ūti-kṛmika-karṇayoḥ
vami-pūrvā hitā karṇa-vidradhau vidradhi-kriyā ।
pittottha-karṇa-śūloktaṃ kartavyaṃ kṣata-vidradhau ।।

amiḥ pūrvaṃ hitā karṇa-
arśo-'rbudeṣu nāsā-vad āmā karṇa-vidārikā ।
karṇa-vidradhi-vat sādhyā yathā-doṣodayena ca ।।

pālī-śoṣe anila-śrotra-śūla-van nasya-lepanam ।
svedaṃ ca kuryāt svinnāṃ ca pālīm udvartayet tilaiḥ ।।

priyāla-bīja-yaṣṭy-āhva-hayagandhā-yavānvitaiḥ ।
tataḥ puṣṭi-karaiḥ snehair abhyaṅgaṃ nityam ācaret ।।

śatāvarī-vājigandhā-payasyairaṇḍa-jīvakaiḥ ।
tailaṃ vipakvaṃ sa-kṣīraṃ pālīnāṃ puṣṭi-kṛt param ।।

kalkena jīvanīyena tailaṃ payasi pācitam ।
ānūpa-māṃsa-kvāthe ca pālī-poṣaṇa-vardhanam ।।

ānūpa-māṃsa-kvāthena
pālīṃ chittvāti-saṃkṣīṇāṃ śeṣāṃ saṃdhāya poṣayet ।
yāpyaivaṃ tantrikākhyāpi paripoṭe apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।।

utpāte śītalair lepo jalauko-hṛta-śoṇite ।
jambv-āmra-pallava-balā-yaṣṭī-lodhra-tilotpalaiḥ ।।

sa-dhānyāmlaiḥ sa-mañjiṣṭhaiḥ sa-kadambaiḥ sa-śārivaiḥ ।
siddham abhyañjane tailaṃ visarpokta-ghṛtāni ca ।।

iddham abhyañjanaṃ tailaṃ
unmanthe abhyañjanaṃ tailaṃ godhā-karka-vasānvitam ।
tālapattry-aśvagandhārka-vākucī-phala-saindhavaiḥ ।।

odhā-karki-vasānvitam -vākucī-tila-saindhavaiḥ
surasā-lāṅgalībhyāṃ ca siddhaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca nāvanam ।
dur-viddhe aśmanta-jambv-āmra-pattra-kvāthena secitām ।।

iddhaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ tu nāvanam
tailena pālīṃ sv-abhyaktāṃ su-ślakṣṇair avacūrṇayet ।
cūrṇair madhuka-mañjiṣṭhā-prapuṇḍrāhva-niśodbhavaiḥ ।।

-prapauṇḍrāhva-niśodbhavaiḥ -pauṇḍarīka-niśodbhavaiḥ
lākṣā-viḍaṅga-siddhaṃ ca tailam abhyañjane hitam ।
svinnāṃ go-maya-jaiḥ piṇḍair bahu-śaḥ parilehikām ।।

viḍaṅga-sārair ālimped urabhrī-mūtra-kalkitaiḥ ।
kauṭajeṅguda-kārañja-bīja-śamyāka-valkalaiḥ ।।

atha-vābhyañjanaṃ tair vā kaṭu-tailaṃ vipācayet ।
sa-nimba-pattra-marica-madanair lehikā-vraṇe ।।

chinnaṃ tu karṇaṃ śuddhasya bandham ālocya yaugikam ।
śuddhāsraṃ lāgayel lagne sadyaś-chinne viśodhanam ।।

amyak-chinne viśodhanam
atha grathitvā keśāntaṃ kṛtvā chedana-lekhanam ।
niveśya saṃdhiṃ suṣamaṃ na nimnaṃ na samunnatam ।।

abhyajya madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ picu-plotāvaguṇṭhitam ।
sūtreṇā-gāḍha-śithilaṃ baddhvā cūrṇair avākiret ।।

śoṇita-sthāpanair vraṇyam ācāraṃ cādiśet tataḥ ।
saptāhād āma-tailāktaṃ śanair apanayet picum ।।

śoṇitāsthāpanair vraṇyam
su-rūḍhaṃ jāta-romāṇaṃ śliṣṭa-saṃdhiṃ samaṃ sthiram ।
su-varṣmāṇam a-rogaṃ ca śanaiḥ karṇaṃ vivardhayet ।।

u-varṣmāṇaṃ su-romaṃ ca
jala-śūkaḥ svayaṅguptā rajanyau bṛhatī-phalam ।
aśvagandhā-balā-hasti-pippalī-gaura-sarṣapāḥ ।।

mūlaṃ kośātakāśvaghna-rūpikā-saptaparṇa-jam ।
chucchundarī kāla-mṛtā gṛhaṃ madhu-karī-kṛtam ।।

jatūkā jala-janmā ca tathā śabarakandakam ।
ebhiḥ kalkaiḥ kharaṃ pakvaṃ sa-tailaṃ māhiṣaṃ ghṛtam ।।

athā śabarakandakaḥ
hasty-aśva-mūtreṇa param abhyaṅgāt karṇa-vardhanam ।
atha kuryād vayaḥ-sthasya cchinnāṃ śuddhasya nāsikām ।।

chindyān nāsā-samaṃ pattraṃ tat-tulyaṃ ca kapolataḥ ।
tvaṅ-māṃsaṃ nāsikāsanne rakṣaṃs tat tanu-tāṃ nayet ।।

sīvyed gaṇḍaṃ tataḥ sūcyā sevinyā picu-yuktayā ।
nāsā-cchede atha likhite parivartyopari tvacam ।।

āsā-cchede su-likhite
kapola-vadhraṃ saṃdadhyāt sīvyen nāsāṃ ca yatnataḥ ।
nāḍībhyām utkṣiped antaḥ sukhocchvāsa-pravṛttaye ।।

apola-bandhaṃ saṃdadhyāt apola-vadhrīṃ saṃdadhyāt
āma-tailena siktvānu pattaṅga-madhukāñjanaiḥ ।
śoṇita-sthāpanaiś cānyaiḥ su-ślakṣṇair avacūrṇayet ।।

ataṅga-madhukāñjanaiḥ śoṇitāsthāpanaiś cānyaiḥ
tato madhu-ghṛtābhyaktaṃ baddhvācārikam ādiśet ।
jñātvāvasthāntaraṃ kuryāt sadyo-vraṇa-vidhiṃ tataḥ ।।

addhvācāram athādiśet
chindyād rūḍhe adhikaṃ māṃsaṃ nāsopāntāc ca carma tat ।
sīvyet tataś ca su-ślakṣṇaṃ hīnaṃ saṃvardhayet punaḥ ।।

āsopāntāc ca carma-vat
niveśite yathā-nyāsaṃ sadyaś-chinne apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।
nāḍī-yogād vinauṣṭhasya nāsā-saṃdhāna-vad vidhiḥ ।।

adyaś-chede apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ

uttarasthāna
avaśyāyānila-rajo-bhāṣyāti-svapna-jāgaraiḥ ।
nīcāty-uccopadhānena pītenānyena vāriṇā ।।

aty-ambu-pāna-ramaṇa-cchardi-bāṣpa-grahādibhiḥ ।
kruddhā vātolbaṇā doṣā nāsāyāṃ styāna-tāṃ gatāḥ ।।

ṣubdhā vātolbaṇā doṣā ṛddhā vātolbaṇā doṣā
janayanti pratiśyāyaṃ vardhamānaṃ kṣaya-pradam ।
tatra vātāt pratiśyāye mukha-śoṣo bhṛśaṃ kṣavaḥ ।।

ghrāṇoparodha-nistoda-danta-śaṅkha-śiro-vyathāḥ ।
kīṭikā iva sarpantīr manyate parito bhruvau ।।

īṭakā iva sarpanti
svara-sādaś cirāt pākaḥ śiśirāccha-kapha-srutiḥ ।
pittāt tṛṣṇā-jvara-ghrāṇa-piṭikā-saṃbhava-bhramāḥ ।।

ittāt tṛṣṇā-jvaro ghrāṇe iṭikā-saṃbhava-bhramāḥ
nāsāgra-pāko rūkṣoṣṇa-tāmra-pīta-kapha-srutiḥ ।
kaphāt kāso a-ruciḥ śvāso vamathur gātra-gauravam ।।

mādhuryaṃ vadane kaṇḍūḥ snigdha-śukla-kapha-srutiḥ ।
sarva-jo lakṣaṇaiḥ sarvair a-kasmād vṛddhi-śānti-mān ।।

nigdha-śukla-ghana-srutiḥ nigdha-śukla-ghanā srutiḥ
duṣṭaṃ nāsā-sirāḥ prāpya pratiśyāyaṃ karoty asṛk ।
urasaḥ supta-tā tāmra-netra-tvaṃ śvāsa-pūti-tā ।।

kaṇḍūḥ śrotrākṣi-nāsāsu pittoktaṃ cātra lakṣaṇam ।
sarva eva pratiśyāyā duṣṭa-tāṃ yānty upekṣitāḥ ।।

ittotthaṃ cātra lakṣaṇam
yathoktopadravādhikyāt sa sarvendriya-tāpanaḥ ।
sāgni-sāda-jvara-śvāsa-kāsoraḥ-pārśva-vedanaḥ ।।

kupyaty a-kasmād bahu-śo mukha-daurgandhya-śopha-kṛt ।
nāsikā-kleda-saṃśoṣa-śuddhi-rodha-karo muhuḥ ।।

ukha-daurgandhya-śoṣa-kṛt
pūyopamāsitā-rakta-grathita-śleṣma-saṃsrutiḥ ।
mūrchanti cātra kṛmayo dīrgha-snigdha-sitāṇavaḥ ।।

ūyopamāsitā raktā -grathitā śleṣma-saṃsrutiḥ 
grathita-śleṣma-saṃsrutiḥ
pakva-liṅgāni teṣv aṅga-lāghavaṃ kṣavathoḥ śamaḥ ।
śleṣmā sa-cikkaṇaḥ pīto a-jñānaṃ ca rasa-gandhayoḥ ।।

ñānaṃ ca rasa-gandhayoḥ
tīkṣṇāghrāṇopayogārka-raśmi-sūtra-tṛṇādibhiḥ ।
vāta-kopibhir anyair vā nāsikā-taruṇāsthani ।।

īkṣṇa-ghrāṇopayogārka-
vighaṭṭite anilaḥ kruddho ruddhaḥ śṛṅgāṭakaṃ vrajet ।
nivṛttaḥ kurute aty-arthaṃ kṣavathuṃ sa bhṛśa-kṣavaḥ ।।

uddhaḥ śṛṅgāṭakaṃ vrajan ṣavathuṃ sa bhṛśaṅ-kṣavaḥ
śoṣayan nāsikā-srotaḥ kaphaṃ ca kurute anilaḥ ।
śūka-pūrṇābha-nāsā-tvaṃ kṛcchrād ucchvasanaṃ tataḥ ।।

śoṣayen nāsikā-srotaḥ śūka-pūrṇābha-kaṇṭha-tvaṃ 
śūka-pūrṇābha-nāsa-tvaṃ
smṛto asau nāsikā-śoṣo nāsānāhe tu jāyate ।
naddha-tvam iva nāsāyāḥ śleṣma-ruddhena vāyunā ।।

niḥśvāsocchvāsa-saṃrodhāt srotasī saṃvṛte iva ।
pacen nāsā-puṭe pittaṃ tvaṅ-māṃsaṃ dāha-śūla-vat ।।

sa ghrāṇa-pākaḥ srāvas tu tat-saṃjñaḥ śleṣma-saṃbhavaḥ ।
accho jalopamo ajasraṃ viśeṣān niśi jāyate ।।

kaphaḥ pravṛddho nāsāyāṃ ruddhvā srotāṃsy a-pīnasam ।
kuryāt sa-ghurghura-śvāsaṃ pīnasādhika-vedanam ।।

uddhaḥ srotaḥsu pīnasam
aver iva sravaty asya praklinnā tena nāsikā ।
ajasraṃ picchilaṃ pītaṃ pakvaṃ siṅghāṇakaṃ ghanam ।।

raktena nāsā dagdheva bāhyāntaḥ-sparśanā-sahā ।
bhaved dhūmopamocchvāsā sā dīptir dahatīva ca ।।

tālu-mūle malair duṣṭair māruto mukha-nāsikāt ।
śleṣmā ca pūtir nirgacchet pūti-nāsaṃ vadanti tam ।।

nicayād abhighātād vā pūyāsṛṅ nāsikā sravet ।
tat pūya-raktam ākhyātaṃ śiro-dāha-rujā-karam ।।

pitta-śleṣmāvaruddho antar nāsāyāṃ śoṣayen marut ।
kaphaṃ sa śuṣkaḥ puṭa-tāṃ prāpnoti puṭakaṃ tu tat ।।

aphaṃ sa śuṣka-puṭa-tāṃ
arśo-'rbudāni vibhajed doṣa-liṅgair yathā-yatham ।
sarveṣu kṛcchrocchvasanaṃ pīnasaḥ pratataṃ kṣutiḥ ।।

īnasaḥ pratataṃ kṣavaḥ īnasaḥ satataṃ kṣutiḥ
sānunāsika-vādi-tvaṃ pūti-nāsaḥ śiro-vyathā ।
aṣṭā-daśānām ity eṣāṃ yāpayed duṣṭa-pīnasam ।।

ūti-nāsā śiro-vyathā ūtir nāsā śiro-vyathā ṣṭā-daśānām eteṣāṃ āpayed duṣṭa-pīnasān arjayed duṣṭa-pīnasam

uttarasthāna
sarveṣu pīnaseṣv ādau nivātāgāra-go bhajet ।
snehana-sveda-vamana-dhūma-gaṇḍūṣa-dhāraṇam ।।

ivātāgāra-go bhavet
vāso gurūṣṇaṃ śirasaḥ su-ghanaṃ pariveṣṭanam ।
laghv-amla-lavaṇaṃ snigdham uṣṇaṃ bhojanam a-dravam ।।

aghv-amla-lavaṇa-snigdham aghv amlaṃ lavaṇaṃ snigdham
dhanva-māṃsa-guḍa-kṣīra-caṇaka-tri-kaṭūtkaṭam ।
yava-godhūma-bhūyiṣṭhaṃ dadhi-dāḍima-sārikam ।।

adhi-dāḍima-sādhitam
bāla-mūlaka-jo yūṣaḥ kulatthotthaś ca pūjitaḥ ।
kavoṣṇaṃ daśa-mūlāmbu jīrṇāṃ vā vāruṇīṃ pibet ।।

jighrec coraka-tarkārī-vacājājy-upakuñcikāḥ ।
vyoṣa-tālīśa-cavikā-tintiḍīkāmla-vetasam ।।

manaḥśilā-viḍaṅgāla-vacā-tri-kaṭu-hiṅgubhiḥ ।
cūrṇī-kṛtya samāghrātaḥ pratiśyāyo vinaśyati ।।
tad-vad doraka-vally-elā-lavā-tārkṣya-dvi-jīrakaiḥ ।।
sāgny-ajāji dvi-palikaṃ tvag-elā-pattra-pādikam ।
jīrṇād guḍāt tulārdhena pakvena vaṭakī-kṛtam ।।

pīnasa-śvāsa-kāsa-ghnaṃ ruci-svara-karaṃ param ।
śatāhvā-tvag-balā mūlaṃ śyoṇākairaṇḍa-bilva-jam ।।

sāragvadhaṃ pibed dhūmaṃ vasājya-madanānvitam ।
atha-vā sa-ghṛtān saktūn kṛtvā mallaka-saṃpuṭe ।।

tyajet snānaṃ śucaṃ krodhaṃ bhṛśaṃ śayyāṃ himaṃ jalam ।
pibed vāta-pratiśyāye sarpir vāta-ghna-sādhitam ।।

paṭu-pañcaka-siddhaṃ vā vidāry-ādi-gaṇena vā ।
sveda-nasyādikāṃ kuryāt cikitsām arditoditām ।।

pitta-raktotthayoḥ peyaṃ sarpir madhurakaiḥ śṛtam ।
pariṣekān pradehāṃś ca śītaiḥ kurvīta śītalān ।।

dhava-tvak-tri-phalā-śyāmā-śrīparṇī-yaṣṭi-tilvakaiḥ ।
kṣīre daśa-guṇe tailaṃ nāvanaṃ sa-niśaiḥ pacet ।।

-śrīparṇī-yaṣṭi-bilvakaiḥ
kapha-je laṅghanaṃ lepaḥ śiraso gaura-sarṣapaiḥ ।
sa-kṣāraṃ vā ghṛtam pītvā vamet piṣṭais tu nāvanam ।।

a-kṣāraṃ ca ghṛtaṃ pītvā a-kṣāraṃ tu ghṛtaṃ pītvā
bastāmbunā paṭu-vyoṣa-vella-vatsaka-jīrakaiḥ ।
kaṭu-tīkṣṇair ghṛtair nasyaiḥ kavaḍaiḥ sarva-jaṃ jayet ।।

yakṣma-kṛmi-kramaṃ kurvan yāpayed duṣṭa-pīnasam ।
vyoṣorubūka-kṛmijid-dāru-mādrī-gadeṅgudam ।।

akṣma-kṛmi-kramaṃ kuryāt -dāru-mādry-ambudeṅgudam
vārtāka-bījaṃ trivṛtā siddhārthaḥ pūti-matsyakaḥ ।
agnimanthasya puṣpāṇi pīlu-śigru-phalāni ca ।।

aśva-viḍ-rasa-mūtrābhyāṃ hasti-mūtreṇa caikataḥ ।
kṣauma-garbhāṃ kṛtāṃ vartiṃ dhūmaṃ ghrāṇāsyataḥ pibet ।।

kṣavathau puṭakākhye ca tīkṣṇaiḥ pradhamanaṃ hitam ।
śuṇṭhī-kuṣṭha-kaṇā-vella-drākṣā-kalka-kaṣāya-vat ।।

sādhitaṃ tailam ājyaṃ vā nasyaṃ kṣava-puṭa-praṇut ।
nāsā-śoṣe balā-tailaṃ pānādau bhojanaṃ rasaiḥ ।।

snigdho dhūmas tathā svedo nāsānāhe apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।
pāke dīptau ca pitta-ghnaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ nasyādi saṃsrutau ।।

īkṣṇaṃ nasyādi śasyate
kapha-pīnasa-vat pūti-nāsā-pīnasayoḥ kriyā ।
lākṣā-karañja-marica-vella-hiṅgu-kaṇā-guḍaiḥ ।।

avi-mūtra-drutair nasyaṃ kārayed vamane kṛte ।
śigru-siṃhī-nikumbhānāṃ bījaiḥ sa-vyoṣa-saindhavaiḥ ।।

sa-vella-surasais tailaṃ nāvanaṃ paramaṃ hitam ।
pūya-rakte nave kuryād rakta-pīnasa-vat kramam ।।

akta-pīnasa-vat kriyām
ati-pravṛddhe nāḍī-vad dagdheṣv arśo-'rbudeṣu ca ।
nikumbha-kumbha-sindhūttha-manohvāla-kaṇāgnikaiḥ ।।

agdheṣv arśo-'rbudeṣu tu
kalkitair ghṛta-madhv-aktāṃ ghrāṇe vartiṃ praveśayet ।
śigrv-ādi-nāvanaṃ cātra pūti-nāsoditaṃ bhajet ।।

alkitair ghṛta-madhv-āktāṃ

uttarasthāna
mātsya-māhiṣa-vārāha-piśitāmaka-mūlakam ।
māṣa-sūpa-dadhi-kṣīra-śuktekṣu-rasa-phāṇitam ।।

atsya-māhiṣa-vārāha-
avāk-śayyāṃ ca bhajato dviṣato danta-dhāvanam ।
dhūma-cchardana-gaṇḍūṣān ucitaṃ ca sirā-vyadham ।।

kruddhāḥ śleṣmolbaṇā doṣāḥ kurvanty antar mukhaṃ gadān ।
tatra khaṇḍauṣṭha ity ukto vātenauṣṭho dvi-dhā kṛtaḥ ।।

urvanty antar-mukhe gadān
oṣṭha-kope tu pavanāt stabdhāv oṣṭhau mahā-rujau ।
dālyete paripāṭyete paruṣāsita-karkaśau ।।

pittāt tīkṣṇa-sahau pītau sarṣapākṛtibhiś citau ।
piṭikābhir bahu-kledāv āśu-pākau kaphāt punaḥ ।।

iṭikābhir mahā-kledāv
śītā-sahau gurū śūnau sa-varṇa-piṭikācitau ।
saṃnipātād anekābhau dur-gandhāsrāva-picchilau ।।

ur-gandha-srāva-picchilau ur-gandhāv ati-picchilau
a-kasmān mlāna-saṃśūna-rujau viṣama-pākinau ।
raktopasṛṣṭau rudhiraṃ sravataḥ śoṇita-prabhau ।।

kharjūra-sadṛśaṃ cātra kṣīṇe rakte arbudaṃ bhavet ।
māṃsa-piṇḍopamau māṃsāt syātāṃ mūrchat-kṛmī kramāt ।।

tailābha-śvayathu-kledau sa-kaṇḍvau medasā mṛdū ।
kṣata-jāv avadīryete pāṭyete cā-sakṛt punaḥ ।।

a-kaṇḍū medasā mṛdū āṭyete vā-sakṛt punaḥ
grathitau ca punaḥ syātāṃ kaṇḍūlau daśana-cchadau ।
jala-budbuda-vad vāta-kaphād oṣṭhe jalārbudam ।।

gaṇḍālajī sthiraḥ śopho gaṇḍe dāha-jvarānvitaḥ ।
vātād uṣṇa-sahā dantāḥ śīta-sparśe adhika-vyathāḥ ।।

dālyanta iva śūlena śītākhyo dālanaś ca saḥ ।
danta-harṣe pravātāmla-śīta-bhakṣā-kṣamā dvi-jāḥ ।।

-śīta-bhakṣyā-sahā dvi-jāḥ
bhavanty amlāśaneneva sa-rujāś calitā iva ।
danta-bhede dvi-jās toda-bheda-ruk-sphuṭanānvitāḥ ।।

a-rujaś calitā iva -bheda-ruk-vedanānvitāḥ
cālaś caladbhir daśanair bhakṣaṇād adhika-vyathaiḥ ।
karālas tu karālānāṃ daśanānāṃ samudgamaḥ ।।

aśanānāṃ samudbhavaḥ aśanānāṃ samudbhave
danto adhiko adhi-dantākhyaḥ sa coktaḥ khalu vardhanaḥ ।
jāyamāne ati-rug dante jāte tatra tu śāmyati ।।

āyate jāyamāne ati ug jāte tatra śāmyati
a-dhāvanān malo dante kapho vā vāta-śoṣitaḥ ।
pūti-gandhiḥ sthirī-bhūtaḥ śarkarā sāpy upekṣitā ।।

ūti-gandhaḥ sthirī-bhūtaḥ śarkarā so apy upekṣitaḥ
śātayaty aṇu-śo dantāt kapālāni kapālikā ।
śyāvaḥ śyāva-tvam āyāto rakta-pittānilair dvi-jaḥ ।।

śātayaty aṇu-śo danta- -kapālāni kapālikā śyāvaḥ śyāva-tvam āyātā 
akta-pittānilair dvi-jāḥ
sa-mūlaṃ dantam āśritya doṣair ulbaṇa-mārutaiḥ ।
śoṣite majjñi suṣire dante anna-mala-pūrite ।।

pūti-tvāt kṛmayaḥ sūkṣmā jāyante jāyate tataḥ ।
a-hetu-tīvrārti-śamaḥ sa-saṃrambho asitaś calaḥ ।।

pralūnaḥ pūya-rakta-srut sa coktaḥ kṛmi-dantakaḥ ।
śleṣma-raktena pūtīni vahanty asram a-hetukam ।।

rabhūta-pūya-rakta-srut
śīryante danta-māṃsāni mṛdu-klinnāsitāni ca ।
śītādo asāv upa-kuśaḥ pākaḥ pittāsṛg-udbhavaḥ ।।

danta-māṃsāni dahyante raktāny utsedha-vanty ataḥ ।
kaṇḍū-manti sravanty asram ādhmāyante asṛji sthite ।।

calā manda-rujo dantāḥ pūti vaktraṃ ca jāyate ।
dantayos triṣu vā śopho badarāsthi-nibho ghanaḥ ।।

kaphāsrāt tīvra-ruk śīghraṃ pacyate danta-puppuṭaḥ ।
danta-māṃse malaiḥ sāsrair bāhyāntaḥ śvayathur guruḥ ।।

sa-rug-dāhaḥ sraved bhinnaḥ pūyāsraṃ danta-vidradhiḥ ।
śvayathur danta-mūleṣu rujā-vān pitta-rakta-jaḥ ।।

ūyāsre danta-vidradhiḥ
lālā-srāvī sa suṣiro danta-māṃsa-praśātanaḥ ।
sa saṃnipātāj jvara-vān sa-pūya-rudhira-srutiḥ ।।

a saṃnipāta-jvara-vān
mahā-suṣira ity ukto viśīrṇa-dvi-ja-bandhanaḥ ।
dantānte kīla-vac chopho hanu-karṇa-rujā-karaḥ ।।

iśīrṇa-rada-bandhanaḥ
pratihanty abhyavahṛtim śleṣmaṇā so adhi-māṃsakaḥ ।
ghṛṣṭeṣu danta-māṃseṣu saṃrambho jāyate mahān ।।

yasmiṃś calanti dantāś ca sa vidarbho abhighāta-jaḥ ।
danta-māṃsāśritān rogān yaḥ sādhyān apy upekṣate ।।

a vaidarbho abhighāta-jaḥ
antas tasyāsravan doṣaḥ sūkṣmāṃ saṃjanayed gatim ।
pūyaṃ muhuḥ sā sravati tvaṅ-māṃsāsthi-prabhedinī ।।

tāḥ punaḥ pañca vijñeyā lakṣaṇaiḥ svair yathoditaiḥ ।
śāka-pattra-kharā suptā sphuṭitā vāta-dūṣitā ।।

jihvā pittāt sa-dāhoṣā raktair māṃsāṅkuraiś citā ।
śālmalī-kaṇṭakābhais tu kaphena bahalā guruḥ ।।

aphena bahulā guruḥ
kapha-pittād adhaḥ śopho jihvā-stambha-kṛd unnataḥ ।
matsya-gandhir bhavet pakvaḥ so alaso māṃsa-śātanaḥ ।।

prabandhane adho jihvāyāḥ śopho jihvāgra-saṃnibhaḥ ।
sāṅkuraḥ kapha-pittāsrair lāloṣā-stambha-vān kharaḥ ।।

ralambano adho jihvāyāḥ
adhi-jihvaḥ sa-ruk-kaṇḍur vākyāhāra-vighāta-kṛt ।
tādṛg evopa-jihvas tu jihvāyā upari sthitaḥ ।।

tālu-māṃse anilād duṣṭe piṭikāḥ sa-rujaḥ kharāḥ ।
bahvyo ghanāḥ srāva-yutās tās tālu-piṭikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

iṭikāḥ sa-rujāḥ kharāḥ ahvyo ghanāḥ srāva-yuktās
tālu-mūle kaphāt sāsrān matsya-vasti-nibho mṛduḥ ।
pralambaḥ picchilaḥ śopho nāsayāhāram īrayan ।।

kaṇṭhoparodha-tṛṭ-kāsa-vami-kṛt gala-śuṇḍikā ।
tālu-madhye ni-ruṅ māṃsaṃ saṃhataṃ tālu-saṃhatiḥ ।।

padmākṛtis tālu-madhye raktāc chvayathur arbudam ।
kacchapaḥ kacchapākāraś cira-vṛddhiḥ kaphād a-ruk ।।

kolābhaḥ śleṣma-medobhyāṃ puppuṭo nī-rujaḥ sthiraḥ ।
pittena pākaḥ pākākhyaḥ pūyāsrāvī mahā-rujaḥ ।।

vāta-pitta-jvarāyāsais tālu-śoṣas tad-āhvayaḥ ।
jihvā-prabandha-jāḥ kaṇṭhe dāruṇā mārga-rodhinaḥ ।।

māṃsāṅkurāḥ śīghra-cayā rohiṇī śīghra-kāriṇī ।
kaṇṭhāsya-śoṣa-kṛd vātāt sā hanu-śrotra-ruk-karī ।।

ohiṇī sāśu-kāriṇī
pittāj jvaroṣā-tṛṇ-moha-kaṇṭha-dhūmāyanānvitā ।
kṣipra-jā kṣipra-pākāti-rāgiṇī sparśanā-sahā ।।

kaphena picchilā pāṇḍur asṛjā sphoṭakācitā ।
taptāṅgāra-nibhā karṇa-ruk-karī pitta-jākṛtiḥ ।।

gambhīra-pākā nicayāt sarva-liṅga-samanvitā ।
doṣaiḥ kapholbaṇaiḥ śophaḥ kola-vad grathitonnataḥ ।।

śūka-kaṇṭaka-vat kaṇṭhe śālūko mārga-rodhanaḥ ।
vṛndo vṛttonnato dāha-jvara-kṛd gala-pārśva-gaḥ ।।

hanu-saṃdhy-āśritaḥ kaṇṭhe kārpāsī-phala-saṃnibhaḥ ।
picchilo manda-ruk śophaḥ kaṭhinas tuṇḍikerikā ।।

arpāsī-phala-saṃnibhaḥ
bāhyāntaḥ śvayathur ghoro gala-mārgārgalopamaḥ ।
galaugho mūrdha-guru-tā-tandrā-lālā-jvara-pradaḥ ।।

valayaṃ nāti-ruk śophas tad-vad evāyatonnataḥ ।
māṃsa-kīlo gale doṣair eko aneko atha-vā alpa-ruk ।।

kṛcchrocchvāsābhyavahṛtiḥ pṛthu-mūlo gilāyukaḥ ।
bhūri-māṃsāṅkura-vṛtā tīvra-tṛḍ-jvara-mūrdha-ruk ।।

ṛthu-mūlo galāyukaḥ
śata-ghnī nicitā vartiḥ śata-ghnīvāti-ruk-karī ।
vyāpta-sarva-galaḥ śīghra-janma-pāko mahā-rujaḥ ।।

śata-ghnī-nicitevāntaḥ śata-ghnī cāti-ruk-karī
pūti-pūya-nibha-srāvī śvayathur gala-vidradhiḥ ।
jihvāvasāne kaṇṭhādāv a-pākaṃ śvayathuṃ malāḥ ।।
janayanti sthiraṃ raktaṃ nī-rujaṃ tad galārbudam ।।
ī-rujaṃ taṃ galārbudam pavana-śleṣma-medobhir gala-gaṇḍo bhaved bahiḥ ।।
vardhamānaḥ sa kālena muṣka-val lambate ati-ruk ।।
uṣka-val lambate ni-ruk
kṛṣṇo aruṇo vā todāḍhyaḥ sa vātāt kṛṣṇa-rāji-mān ।
vṛddhas tālu-gale śoṣaṃ kuryāc ca vi-rasāsya-tām ।।

sthiraḥ sa-varṇaḥ kaṇḍū-mān śīta-sparśo guruḥ kaphāt ।
vṛddhas tālu-gale lepaṃ kuryāc ca madhurāsya-tām ।।

ṛddhas tālu-gale śophaṃ
medasaḥ śleṣma-vad dhāni-vṛddhyoḥ so anuvidhīyate ।
dehaṃ vṛddhaś ca kurute gale śabdaṃ svare alpa-tām ।।

śleṣma-ruddhānila-gatiḥ śuṣka-kaṇṭho hata-svaraḥ ।
tāmyan prasaktaṃ śvasiti yena sa svara-hānilāt ।।

karoti vadanasyāntar vraṇān sarva-saro anilaḥ ।
saṃcāriṇo aruṇān rūkṣān oṣṭhau tāmrau cala-tvacau ।।

jihvā śītā-sahā gurvī sphuṭitā kaṇṭakācitā ।
vivṛṇoti ca kṛcchreṇa mukhaṃ pāko mukhasya saḥ ।।

ukhaṃ pāko mukhasya ca
adhaḥ pratihato vāyur arśo-gulma-kaphādibhiḥ ।
yāty ūrdhvaṃ vaktra-daurgandhyaṃ kurvann ūrdhva-gudas tu saḥ ।।

urvann ūrdhva-gadas tu saḥ
mukhasya pitta-je pāke dāhoṣe tikta-vaktra-tā ।
kṣārokṣita-kṣata-samā vraṇās tad-vac ca rakta-je ।।

kapha-je madhurāsya-tvaṃ kaṇḍū-mat-picchilā vraṇāḥ ।
antaḥ-kapolam āśritya śyāva-pāṇḍu kapho arbudam ।।

śyāvaṃ pāṇḍu kapho arbudam
kuryāt tad ghaṭṭitaṃ chinnaṃ mṛditaṃ ca vivardhate ।
mukha-pāko bhavet sāsraiḥ sarvaiḥ sarvākṛtir malaiḥ ।।

uryāt tat pāṭitaṃ chinnaṃ uryāt tad vyadhitaṃ chinnaṃ
pūty-āsya-tā ca tair eva danta-kāṣṭhādi-vidviṣaḥ ।
oṣṭhe gaṇḍe dvi-je mūle jihvāyāṃ tāluke gale ।।

vaktre sarva-tra cety uktāḥ pañca-saptatir āmayāḥ ।
ekā-daśaiko daśa ca trayo-daśa tathā ca ṣaṭ ।।

aṣṭāv aṣṭā-daśāṣṭau ca kramāt teṣv an-upakramāḥ ।
karālo māṃsa-raktauṣṭhāv arbudāni jalād vinā ।।

ramād eṣv an-upakramāḥ
kacchapas tālu-piṭikā galaughaḥ suṣiro mahān ।
svara-ghnordhva-guda-śyāva-śata-ghnī-valayālasāḥ ।।

vara-ghnordhva-gada-śyāva-
nāḍy-oṣṭha-kopau nicayād raktāt sarvaiś ca rohiṇī ।
daśane sphuṭite danta-bhedaḥ pakvopa-jihvikā ।।

gala-gaṇḍaḥ svara-bhraṃśī kṛcchrocchvāso ati-vatsaraḥ ।
yāpyas tu harṣo bhedaś ca śeṣāñ chastrauṣadhair jayet ।।

ala-gaṇḍaḥ svara-bhraṃśaḥ

uttarasthāna
khaṇḍauṣṭhasya vilikhyāntau syūtvā vraṇa-vad ācaret ।
yaṣṭī-jyotiṣmatī-lodhra-śrāvaṇī-śārivotpalaiḥ ।।

paṭolyā kākamācyā ca tailam abhyañjanaṃ pacet ।
nasyaṃ ca tailaṃ vāta-ghna-madhura-skandha-sādhitam ।।

mahā-snehena vātauṣṭhe siddhenāktaḥ picur hitaḥ ।
deva-dhūpa-madhūcchiṣṭa-guggulv-amaradārubhiḥ ।।

yaṣṭy-āhva-cūrṇa-yuktena tenaiva pratisāraṇam ।
nāḍy-oṣṭhaṃ svedayed dugdha-siddhair eraṇḍa-pallavaiḥ ।।

aṣṭy-āhva-cūrṇa-yuktais tu air eva pratisāraṇam
khaṇḍauṣṭha-vihitaṃ nasyaṃ tasya mūrdhni ca tarpaṇam ।
pittābhighāta-jāv oṣṭhau jalaukobhir upācaret ।।

lodhra-sarja-rasa-kṣaudra-madhukaiḥ pratisāraṇam ।
guḍūcī-yaṣṭi-pattaṅga-siddham abhyañjane ghṛtam ।।

pitta-vidradhi-vac cātra kriyā śoṇita-je api ca ।
idam eva nave kāryaṃ karmauṣṭhe tu kaphāture ।।

dam eva bhavet kāryaṃ armauṣṭhe tu kaphottare
pāṭhā-kṣāra-madhu-vyoṣair hṛtāsre pratisāraṇam ।
dhūma-nāvana-gaṇḍūṣāḥ prayojyāś ca kapha-cchidaḥ ।।

svinnaṃ bhinnaṃ vi-medaskaṃ dahen medo-jam agninā ।
priyaṅgu-lodhra-tri-phalā-mākṣikaiḥ pratisārayet ।।

sa-kṣaudrā gharṣaṇaṃ tīkṣṇā bhinna-śuddhe jalārbude ।
avagāḍhe ati-vṛddhe vā kṣāro agnir vā pratikriyā ।।

a-kṣaudrair gharṣaṇaṃ tīkṣṇair ṣāro vahniḥ pratikriyā
āmādy-avasthāsv alajīṃ gaṇḍe śopha-vad ācaret ।
svinnasya śīta-dantasya pālīṃ vilikhitāṃ dahet ।।

tailena pratisāryā ca sa-kṣaudra-ghana-saindhavaiḥ ।
dāḍima-tvag-varā-tārkṣya-kāntā-jambv-asthi-nāgaraiḥ ।।

kavaḍaḥ kṣīriṇāṃ kvāthair aṇu-tailaṃ ca nāvanam ।
danta-harṣe tathā bhede sarvā vāta-harā kriyā ।।

anta-bhede tathā harṣe arvā vāta-harāḥ kriyāḥ
tila-yaṣṭīmadhu-śṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ gaṇḍūṣa-dhāraṇam ।
sa-snehaṃ daśa-mūlāmbu gaṇḍūṣaḥ pracalad-dvi-je ।।

a-sneha-daśa-mūlāmbu- -gaṇḍūṣāḥ pracale dvi-je
tuttha-lodhra-kaṇā-śreṣṭhā-pattaṅga-paṭu-gharṣaṇam ।
snigdhāḥ śīlyā yathāvasthaṃ nasyānna-kavaḍādayaḥ ।।

aṇḍūṣa-kavaḍādayaḥ
adhi-dantakam āliptaṃ yadā kṣāreṇa jarjaram ।
kṛmi-dantam ivotpāṭya tad-vac copacaret tadā ।।

an-avasthita-rakte ca dagdhe vraṇa iva kriyā ।
a-hiṃsan danta-mūlāni dantebhyaḥ śarkarāṃ haret ।।

kṣāra-cūrṇair madhu-yutais tataś ca pratisārayet ।
kapālikāyām apy evaṃ harṣoktaṃ ca samācaret ।।

jayed visrāvaṇaiḥ svinnam a-calaṃ kṛmi-dantakam ।
snigdhaiś cālepa-gaṇḍūṣa-nasyāhāraiś calāpahaiḥ ।।

-balaṃ kṛmi-dantakam
guḍena pūrṇaṃ suṣiraṃ madhūcchiṣṭena vā dahet ।
saptacchadārka-kṣīrābhyāṃ pūraṇaṃ kṛmi-śūla-jit ।।

hiṅgu-kaṭphala-kāsīsa-svarjikā-kuṣṭha-vella-jam ।
rajo rujaṃ jayaty āśu vastra-sthaṃ daśane ghṛtam ।।

astra-sthaṃ daśanair ghṛtam
alaktakaṃ vā sindhūtthaṃ vella-dhūmaṃ sa-hiṅgu vā ।
dhānyāmla-siddhaṃ śevālaṃ koṣṇaṃ vā daśana-sthitam ।।

eśma-dhūmaṃ sa-hiṅgu vā
varāhakarṇī-mūlaṃ vā śarapuṅkhā-jaṭātha-vā ।
vartir vāvalguja-phalair bījapūra-jaṭānvitaiḥ ।।

gaṇḍūṣaṃ grāhayet tailam ebhir eva ca sādhitam ।
kvāthair vā yuktam eraṇḍa-dvi-vyāghrī-bhūkadamba-jaiḥ ।।

aṇḍūṣaṃ dhārayet tailam -vyāghrī-bhūrja-kadambakaiḥ
kriyā-yogair bahu-vidhair ity a-śānta-rujaṃ bhṛśam ।
dṛḍham apy uddhared dantaṃ pūrvaṃ mūlād vimokṣitam ।।

saṃdaṃśakena laghunā danta-nirghātanena vā ।
tailaṃ sa-yaṣṭy-āhva-rajo gaṇḍūṣo madhu vā tataḥ ।।

aṇḍūṣo madhunā tataḥ
tato vidāri-yaṣṭy-āhva-śṛṅgāṭaka-kaserubhiḥ ।
tailaṃ daśa-guṇa-kṣīraṃ siddhaṃ yuñjīta nāvanam ।।

kṛśa-dur-bala-vṛddhānāṃ vātārtānāṃ ca noddharet ।
noddharec cottaraṃ dantaṃ bahūpadrava-kṛd dhi saḥ ।।

eṣām apy uddhṛtau snigdha-svādu-śīta-kramo hitaḥ ।
visrāvitāsre śītāde sa-kṣaudraiḥ pratisāraṇam ।।

ṣām apy uddhṛtaiḥ snigdha-
mustārjuna-tvak-tri-phalā-phalinī-tārkṣya-nāgaraiḥ ।
tat-kvāthaḥ kavaḍo nasyaṃ tailaṃ madhura-sādhitam ।।

danta-māṃsāny upa-kuśe svinnāny uṣṇāmbu-dhāraṇaiḥ ।
maṇḍalāgreṇa śākādi-pattrair vā bahu-śo likhet ।।

tataś ca pratisāryāṇi ghṛta-maṇḍa-madhu-drutaiḥ ।
lākṣā-priyaṅgu-pattaṅga-lavaṇottama-gairikaiḥ ।।

hṛta-maṇḍa-madhu-plutaiḥ
sa-kuṣṭha-śuṇṭhī-marica-yaṣṭīmadhu-rasāñjanaiḥ ।
sukhoṣṇo ghṛta-maṇḍo anu tailaṃ vā kavaḍa-grahaḥ ।।

ailaṃ vā kavaḍa-grahe
ghṛtaṃ ca madhuraiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ kavaḍa-nasyayoḥ ।
danta-puppuṭake svinna-cchinna-bhinna-vilekhite ।।

hṛtaṃ vā madhuraiḥ siddhaṃ
yaṣṭy-āhva-svarjikā-śuṇṭhī-saindhavaiḥ pratisāraṇam ।
vidradhau kaṭu-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-rūkṣaiḥ kavaḍa-lepanam ।।

gharṣaṇaṃ kaṭukā-kuṣṭha-vṛścikālī-yavodbhavaiḥ ।
rakṣet pākaṃ himaiḥ pakvaḥ pāṭyo dāhyo avagāḍhakaḥ ।।

suṣire chinna-likhite sa-kṣaudraiḥ pratisāraṇam ।
lodhra-musta-miśi-śreṣṭhā-tārkṣya-pattaṅga-kiṃśukaiḥ ।।

auṣire chinna-likhite
sa-kaṭphalaiḥ kaṣāyaiś ca teṣāṃ gaṇḍūṣa iṣyate ।
yaṣṭī-lodhrotpalānantā-śārivāguru-candanaiḥ ।।

a-kaṭphalaiḥ kaṣāyaś ca
sa-gairika-sitā-puṇḍraiḥ siddhaṃ tailaṃ ca nāvanam ।
chittvādhi-māṃsakaṃ cūrṇaiḥ sa-kṣaudraiḥ pratisārayet ।।

vacā-tejovatī-pāṭhā-svarjikā-yava-śūka-jaiḥ ।
paṭola-nimba-tri-phalā-kaṣāyaḥ kavaḍo hitaḥ ।।

-svarjikā-yāva-śūka-jaiḥ
vidarbhe danta-mūlāni maṇḍalāgreṇa śodhayet ।
kṣāraṃ yuñjyāt tato nasyaṃ gaṇḍūṣādi ca śītalam ।।

saṃśodhyobhayataḥ kāyaṃ śiraś copacaret tataḥ ।
nāḍīṃ dantānugāṃ dantaṃ samuddhṛtyāgninā dahet ।।

kubjāṃ naika-gatiṃ pūrṇāṃ guḍena madanena vā ।
dhāvanaṃ jāti-madana-khadira-svādukaṇṭakaiḥ ।।

yubjāṃ naika-gatiṃ pūrṇāṃ uḍena madhunātha-vā
kṣīri-vṛkṣāmbu-gaṇḍūṣo nasyaṃ tailaṃ ca tat-kṛtam ।
kuryād vātauṣṭha-kopoktaṃ kaṇṭakeṣv anilātmasu ।।

jihvāyāṃ pitta-jāteṣu ghṛṣṭeṣu rudhire srute ।
pratisāraṇa-gaṇḍūṣa-nāvanaṃ madhurair hitam ।।

tīkṣṇaiḥ kaphottheṣv evaṃ ca sarṣapa-try-ūṣaṇādibhiḥ ।
nave jihvālase apy evaṃ taṃ tu śastreṇa na spṛśet ।।

īkṣṇaiḥ kaphottheṣv apy evaṃ īkṣṇaiḥ kaphottheṣv evaṃ tu
unnamya jihvām ākṛṣṭāṃ baḍiśenādhi-jihvikām ।
chedayen maṇḍalāgreṇa tīkṣṇoṣṇair gharṣaṇādi ca ।।

upa-jihvāṃ parisrāvya yava-kṣāreṇa gharṣayet ।
kapha-ghnaiḥ śuṇḍikā sādhyā nasya-gaṇḍūṣa-gharṣaṇaiḥ ।।

ervāru-bīja-pratimaṃ vṛddhāyām a-sirā-tatam ।
agraṃ niviṣṭaṃ jihvāyā baḍīśādy-avalambitam ।।

graṃ niviṣṭaṃ jihvāyāṃ gre niviṣṭaṃ jihvāyā
chedayen maṇḍalāgreṇa nāty-agre na ca mūlataḥ ।
chede aty asṛk-kṣayān mṛtyur hīne vyādhir vivardhate ।।

āty-agre nāti-mūlataḥ
maricātiviṣā-pāṭhā-vacā-kuṣṭha-kuṭannaṭaiḥ ।
chinnāyāṃ sa-paṭu-kṣaudrair gharṣaṇaṃ kavaḍaḥ punaḥ ।।

kaṭukātiviṣā-pāṭhā-nimba-rāsnā-vacāmbubhiḥ ।
saṃghāte puppuṭe kūrme vilikhyaivaṃ samācaret ।।

a-pakve tālu-pāke tu kāsīsa-kṣaudra-tārkṣya-jaiḥ ।
gharṣaṇaṃ kavaḍaḥ śīta-kaṣāya-madhurauṣadhaiḥ ।।

harṣaṇaṃ kavaḍaḥ śītaḥ aṣāya-madhurauṣadhaiḥ
pakve aṣṭā-pada-vad bhinne tīkṣṇoṣṇaiḥ pratisāraṇam ।
vṛṣa-nimba-paṭolādyais tiktaiḥ kavaḍa-dhāraṇam ।।

tālu-śoṣe tv a-tṛṣṇasya sarpir uttara-bhaktikam ।
kaṇā-śuṇṭhī-śṛtaṃ pānam amlair gaṇḍūṣa-dhāraṇam ।।

ālu-śoṣe tṛṣārtasya
dhanva-māṃsa-rasāḥ snigdhāḥ kṣīra-sarpiś ca nāvanam ।
kaṇṭha-rogeṣv asṛṅ-mokṣas tīkṣṇair nasyādi karma ca ।।

kvāthaḥ pānaṃ ca dārvī-tvaṅ-nimba-tārkṣya-kaliṅga-jaḥ ।
harītakī-kaṣāyo vā peyo mākṣika-saṃyutaḥ ।।

śreṣṭhā-vyoṣa-yava-kṣāra-dārvī-dvīpi-rasāñjanaiḥ ।
sa-pāṭhā-tejinī-nimbaiḥ śukta-go-mūtra-sādhitaiḥ ।।

kavaḍo guṭikā vātra kalpitā pratisāraṇam ।
niculaṃ kaṭabhī mustaṃ devadāru mahauṣadham ।।

avaḍo guṭikā cātra iculaṃ kaṭabhī mustā
vacā dantī ca mūrvā ca lepaḥ koṣṇo arti-śopha-hā ।
athāntar-bāhyataḥ svinnāṃ vāta-rohiṇikāṃ likhet ।।

aṅgulī-śastrakeṇāśu paṭu-yukta-nakhena vā ।
pañca-mūlāmbu kavaḍas tailaṃ gaṇḍūṣa-nāvanam ।।

visrāvya pitta-saṃbhūtāṃ sitā-kṣaudra-priyaṅgubhiḥ ।
gharṣet sa-lodhra-pattaṅgaiḥ kavaḍaḥ kvathitaiś ca taiḥ ।।

drākṣā-parūṣaka-kvātho hitaś ca kavaḍa-grahe ।
upācared evam eva pratyākhyāyāsra-saṃbhavām ।।

sāgāra-dhūmaiḥ kaṭukaiḥ kapha-jāṃ pratisārayet ।
nasya-gaṇḍūṣayos tailaṃ sādhitaṃ ca praśasyate ।।

apāmārga-phala-śvetā-dantī-jantughna-saindhavaiḥ ।
tad-vac ca vṛnda-śālūka-tuṇḍikerī-gilāyuṣu ।।

-tuṇḍikerī-galāyuṣu
vidradhau srāvite śreṣṭhā-rocanā-tārkṣya-gairikaiḥ ।
sa-lodhra-paṭu-pattaṅga-kaṇair gaṇḍūṣa-gharṣaṇe ।।

-kaṇair gaṇḍūṣa-dhāraṇam -kaṇair gaṇḍūṣa-gharṣaṇam
gala-gaṇḍaḥ pavana-jaḥ svinno niḥsruta-śoṇitaḥ ।
tilair bījaiś ca laṭvomā-priyāla-śaṇa-saṃbhavaiḥ ।।

vinno visruta-śoṇitaḥ
upanāhyo vraṇe rūḍhe pralepyaś ca punaḥ punaḥ ।
śigru-tilvaka-tarkārī-gaja-kṛṣṇā-punarnavaiḥ ।।

kālāmṛtārka-mūlaiś ca puṣpaiś ca karahāṭa-jaiḥ ।
ekaiṣīkānvitaiḥ piṣṭaiḥ surayā kāñjikena vā ।।

āla-mūlārka-mūlaiś ca uṣpaiś ca karaghāṭa-jaiḥ
guḍūcī-nimba-kuṭaja-haṃsapadī-balā-dvayaiḥ ।
sādhitaṃ pāyayet tailaṃ sa-kṛṣṇā-devadārubhiḥ ।।

kartavyaṃ kapha-je apy etat sveda-vimlāpane tv ati ।
lepo ajagandhātiviṣā-viśalyāḥ sa-viṣāṇikāḥ ।।

guñjālābu-śukāhvāś ca palāśa-kṣāra-kalkitāḥ ।
mūtra-srutaṃ haṭha-kṣāraṃ paktvā kodrava-bhuk pibet ।।

ūtra-śṛtaṃ yava-kṣāraṃ ūtra-srutaṃ yava-kṣāraṃ 
sūtra-srutaṃ yava-kṣāraṃ
sādhitaṃ vatsakādyair vā tailaṃ sa-paṭu-pañcakaiḥ ।
kapha-ghnān dhūma-vamana-nāvanādīṃś ca śīlayet ।।

apha-ghnān dhūma-gaṇḍūṣān amanādīṃś ca śīlayet
medo-bhave sirāṃ vidhyet kapha-ghnaṃ ca vidhiṃ bhajet ।
asanādi-rajaś cainaṃ prātar mūtreṇa pāyayet ।।

a-śāntau pācayitvā ca sarvān vraṇa-vad ācaret ।
mukha-pākeṣu sa-kṣaudrā prayojyā mukha-dhāvanāḥ ।।

-śāntau pāṭayitvā ca rayojyā mukha-pāvanāḥ
kvathitās tri-phalā-pāṭhā-mṛdvīkā-jāti-pallavāḥ ।
niṣṭhevyā bhakṣayitvā vā kuṭherādir gaṇo atha-vā ।।

ighṛṣṭavyā bhakṣayitvā
mukha-pāke anilāt kṛṣṇā-paṭv-elāḥ pratisāraṇam ।
tailaṃ vāta-haraiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ kavaḍa-nasyayoḥ ।।

pittāsre pitta-rakta-ghnaḥ kapha-ghnaś ca kaphe vidhiḥ ।
likhec chākādi-pattraiś ca piṭikāḥ kaṭhināḥ sthirāḥ ।।

ittāsre rakta-pitta-ghnaḥ
yathā-doṣodayaṃ kuryāt saṃnipāte cikitsitam ।
nave arbude tv a-saṃvṛddhe chedite pratisāraṇam ।।

svarjikā-nāgara-kṣaudraiḥ kvātho gaṇḍūṣa iṣyate ।
guḍūcī-nimba-kalkottho madhu-taila-samanvitaḥ ।।

yavānna-bhuk tīkṣṇa-taila-nasyābhyaṅgāṃs tathācaret ।
vamite pūti-vadane dhūmas tīkṣṇaḥ sa-nāvanaḥ ।।

samaṅgā-dhātakī-lodhra-phalinī-padmakair jalam ।
dhāvanaṃ vadanasyāntaś cūrṇitair avacūrṇitam ।।

ūrṇitair avacūrṇanam śītādopa-kuśoktaṃ ca nāvanādi ca śīlayet ।।
phala-traya-dvīpi-kirātatikta-yaṣṭy-āhva-siddhārtha-kaṭu-trikāṇi ।।mustā-haridrā-dvaya-yāva-śūka-vṛkṣāmlakāmlāgrima-vetasāś ca ।।
aśvattha-jambv-āmra-dhanañjaya-tvak tvak cāhimārāt khadirasya sāraḥ ।
kvāthena teṣāṃ ghana-tāṃ gatena tac-cūrṇa-yuktā guṭikā vidheyāḥ ।।

tā dhāritā ghnanti mukhena nityaṃ kaṇṭhauṣṭha-tālv-ādi-gadān su-kṛcchrān ।
viśeṣato rohiṇikāsya-śoṣa-gandhān videhādhipati-praṇītāḥ ।।

khadira-tulām ambu-ghaṭe paktvā toyena tena piṣṭaiś ca ।
candana-joṅgaka-kuṅkuma-paripelava-vālakośīraiḥ ।।

surataru-lodhra-drākṣā-mañjiṣṭhā-coca-padmaka-viḍaṅgaiḥ ।
spṛkkā-nata-nakha-kaṭphala-sūkṣmailā-dhyāmakaiḥ sa-pattaṅgaiḥ ।।

taila-prasthaṃ vipacet karṣāṃśaiḥ pāna-nasya-gaṇḍūṣais tat ।
hatvāsye sarva-gadān janayati gārdhrīṃ dṛśaṃ śrutiṃ ca vārāhīm ।।

arṣāṃśaiḥ pāna-nasya-gaṇḍūṣaiḥ anty āsye sarva-gadān
udvartitaṃ ca prapunāṭa-lodhra-dārvībhir abhyaktam anena vaktram ।
nir-vyaṅga-nīlī-mukha-dūṣikādi saṃjāyate candra-samāna-kānti ।।

ir-vyaṅga-nīlī-mukha-dūṣikaṃ ca
pala-śataṃ bāṇāt toya-ghaṭe paktvā rase asmiṃś ca palārdhikaiḥ ।
khadira-jambū-yaṣṭyānantāmrair ahimāra-nīlotpalānvitaiḥ ।।

hadira-jambū-yaṣṭyānantā-lodhrair
taila-prasthaṃ pācayec chlakṣṇa-piṣṭair ebhir dravyair dhāritaṃ tan mukhena ।
rogān sarvān hanti vaktre viśeṣāt sthairyaṃ dhatte danta-paṅkteś calāyāḥ ।।

aila-prasthaṃ pācayet sūkṣma-piṣṭair bhir dravyair dhāritaṃ 
tat sukhena
khadira-sārād dve tule paced valkāt tulāṃ cārimedasaḥ ।
ghaṭa-catuṣke pāda-śeṣe asmin pūte punaḥ kvathanād ghane ।।

hadira-sārād dve tule vipaced alka-tulāṃ cārimedasaḥ alkala-tulāṃ cārimedasaḥ alkala-tulāṃ cārimedataḥ 'smin pūte punaḥ kvāthanād ghane 'smin pūte punaḥ kvāthayed 
ghane
ākṣikaṃ kṣipet su-sūkṣmaṃ rajaḥ sevyāmbu-pattaṅga-gairikam ।
candana-dvaya-lodhra-puṇḍrāhva-yaṣṭy-āhva-lākṣāñjana-dvayam ।।

ākṣikaṃ kṣipet su-sūkṣma-rajaḥ ākṣikaṃ ca kṣipet sūkṣma-rajaḥ ārṣikaṃ kṣipet su-sūkṣma-rajaḥ 
candana-dvaya-śyāmā-puṇḍrāhva-
dhātakī-kaṭphala-dvi-niśā-tri-phalā-catur-jāta-joṅgakam ।
musta-mañjiṣṭhā-nyagrodha-praroha-māṃsī-yavāsakam ।।

ṃdha-praroha-vacā-māṃsī-yavāsakam
padmakailā-samaṅgāś ca śīte tasmiṃs tathā pālikāṃ pṛthak ।
jātīpattrikāṃ sa-jāti-phalāṃ saha-lavaṅga-kaṇkollakām ।।

admakaileya-samaṅgāś ca śīte tathā pālikāṃ pṛthak 
aha-nakha-lavaṅga-kaṅkollakām
sphaṭika-śubhra-surabhi-karpūra-kuḍavaṃ ca tatrāvapet tataḥ ।
kārayed guṭikāḥ sadā caitā dhāryā mukhe tad-gadāpahāḥ ।।

ārayed guṭikāś caitā āryāś caitā guṭikā
kvāthyauṣadha-vyatyaya-yojanena tailaṃ pacet kalpanayānayaiva ।
sarvāsya-rogoddhṛtaye tad āhur danta-sthira-tve tv idam eva mukhyam ।।

vāthauṣadha-vyatyaya-yojanena arvāsya-roga-praśamārtham uktaṃ 
arvāsya-roge vyayanaṃ tad āhur
khadireṇaitā guṭikās tailam idaṃ cārimedasā prathitam ।
anuśīlayan prati-dinaṃ svastho api dṛḍha-dvi-jo bhavati ।।

ṛddho api dṛḍha-dvi-jo bhavati
kṣudrā-guḍūcī-sumanaḥ-pravāla-dārvī-yavāsa-tri-phalā-kaṣāyaḥ ।
kṣaudreṇa yuktaḥ kavaḍa-graho ayaṃ sarvāmayān vaktra-gatān nihanti ।।

rākṣā-guḍūcī-sumanaḥ-pravāla-
pāṭhā-dārvī-tvak-kuṣṭha-mustā-samaṅgā-tiktā-pītāṅgī-lodhra-tejovatīnām ।
cūrṇaḥ sa-kṣaudro danta-māṃsārti-kaṇḍū-pāka-srāvāṇāṃ nāśano gharṣaṇena ।।

gṛha-dhūma-tārkṣya-pāṭhā-vyoṣa-kṣārāgny-ayo-varā-tejo-hvaiḥ ।
mukha-danta-gala-vikāre sa-kṣaudraḥ kālako vidhāryaś cūrṇaḥ ।।

a-kṣaudraḥ kāliko vidhāryaś cūrṇaḥ
dārvī-tvak-sindhūdbhava-manaḥśilā-yāva-śūka-haritālaiḥ ।
dhāryaḥ pītaka-cūrṇo dantāsya-galāmaye sa-madhv-ājyaḥ ।।

dvi-kṣāra-dhūmaka-varā-pañca-paṭu-vyoṣa-vella-giri-tārkṣyaiḥ ।
go-mūtreṇa vipakvā galāmaya-ghnī rasa-kriyā eṣā ।।

vi-kṣāra-gṛha-dhūmaka-varā- o-mūtreṇa piban kvāthaṃ
go-mūtra-kvathana-vilīna-vigrahāṇāṃ pathyānāṃ jala-miśi-kuṣṭha-bhāvitānām ।
attāraṃ naram aṇavo api vaktra-rogāḥ śrotāraṃ nṛpam iva na spṛśanty an-arthāḥ ।।

saptacchadośīra-paṭola-musta-harītakī-tiktaka-rohiṇībhiḥ ।
yaṣṭy-āhva-rājadruma-candanaiś ca kvāthaṃ pibet pāka-haraṃ mukhasya ।।

paṭola-śuṇṭhī-tri-phalā-viśālā-trāyanti-tiktā-dvi-niśāmṛtānām ।
pītaḥ kaṣāyo madhunā nihanti mukhe sthitaś cāsya-gadān a-śeṣān ।।

ukhotthitāṃś cāśu gadān a-śeṣān
sva-rasaḥ kvathito dārvyā ghanī-bhūtaḥ sa-gairikaḥ ।
āsya-sthaḥ sa-madhur vaktra-pāka-nāḍī-vraṇāpahaḥ ।।

paṭola-nimba-yaṣṭy-āhva-vāsā-jāty-arimedasām ।
khadirasya varāyāś ca pṛthag evaṃ prakalpanā ।।

khadirāyo-varā-pārtha-madayanty-ahimārakaiḥ ।
gaṇḍūṣo ambu-śṛtair dhāryo dur-bala-dvi-ja-śāntaye ।।

mukha-danta-mūla-gala-jāḥ prāyo rogāḥ kaphāsra-bhūyiṣṭhāḥ ।
tasmāt teṣām a-sakṛd rudhiraṃ visrāvayed duṣṭam ।।

kāya-śirasor vireko vamanaṃ kavaḍa-grahāś ca kaṭu-tiktāḥ ।
prāyaḥ śastaṃ teṣāṃ kapha-rakta-haraṃ tathā karma ।।

yava-tṛṇa-dhānyaṃ bhaktaṃ vidalaiḥ kṣāroṣitair apa-snehāḥ ।
yūṣā bhakṣyāś ca hitā yac cānyac chleṣma-nāśāya ।।

ava-tṛṇa-dhānyaṃ bhuktaṃ idalaiḥ kṣāroṣitair apa-sneham
prāṇānila-patha-saṃsthāḥ śvasitam api nirundhate pramāda-vataḥ ।
kaṇṭhāmayāś cikitsitam ato drutaṃ teṣu kurvīta ।।

uttarasthāna
dhūmātapa-tuṣārāmbu-krīḍāti-svapna-jāgaraiḥ ।
utsvedādhi-puro-vāta-bāṣpa-nigraha-rodanaiḥ ।।

nmādādhi-puro-vāta-
aty-ambu-madya-pānena kṛmibhir vega-dhāraṇaiḥ ।
upadhāna-mṛjābhyaṅga-dveṣādhaḥ-pratatekṣaṇaiḥ ।।

a-sātmya-gandha-duṣṭāma-bhāṣyādyaiś ca śiro-gatāḥ ।
janayanty āmayān doṣās tatra māruta-kopataḥ ।।

-sātmya-gandha-duṣṭāmbu-
nistudyete bhṛśaṃ śaṅkhau ghāṭā saṃbhidyate tathā ।
bhruvor madhyaṃ lalāṭaṃ ca patatīvāti-vedanam ।।

hruvor madhye lalāṭaṃ ca
bādhyete svanataḥ śrotre niṣkṛṣyete ivākṣiṇī ।
ghūrṇatīva śiraḥ sarvaṃ saṃdhibhya iva mucyate ।।

sphuraty ati sirā-jālaṃ kandharā-hanu-saṃgrahaḥ ।
prakāśā-saha-tā ghrāṇa-srāvo a-kasmād vyathā-śamau ।।

mārdavaṃ mardana-sneha-sveda-bandhaiś ca jāyate ।
śiras-tāpo ayam ardhe tu mūrdhnaḥ so ardhāvabhedakaḥ ।।

pakṣāt kupyati māsād vā svayam eva ca śāmyati ।
ati-vṛddhas tu nayanaṃ śravaṇaṃ vā vināśayet ।।

śiro-'bhitāpe pittotthe śiro-dhūmāyanaṃ jvaraḥ ।
svedo akṣi-dahanaṃ mūrchā niśi śītaiś ca mārdavam ।।

a-ruciḥ kapha-je mūrdhno guru-stimita-śīta-tā ।
sirā-niṣpanda-tālasyaṃ ruṅ mandāhny adhikā niśi ।।

tandrā śūnākṣi-kūṭa-tvaṃ karṇa-kaṇḍūyanaṃ vamiḥ ।
raktāt pittādhika-rujaḥ sarvaiḥ syāt sarva-lakṣaṇaḥ ।।

saṃkīrṇair bhojanair mūrdhni kledite rudhirāmiṣe ।
kopite saṃnipāte ca jāyante mūrdhni jantavaḥ ।।

śirasas te pibanto asraṃ ghorāḥ kurvanti vedanāḥ ।
citta-vibhraṃśa-jananīr jvaraḥ kāso bala-kṣayaḥ ।।

raukṣya-śopha-vyadha-ccheda-dāha-sphuraṇa-pūti-tāḥ ।
kapāle tālu-śirasoḥ kaṇḍūḥ śoṣaḥ pramīlakaḥ ।।

aukṣya-śophe vyadha-ccheda- -dāha-sphuṭana-pūti-tāḥ 
aṇḍūḥ śophaḥ pramīlakaḥ aṇḍūḥ śopho a-pramīlakaḥ
tāmrāccha-siṅghāṇaka-tā karṇa-nādaś ca jantu-je ।
vātolbaṇāḥ śiraḥ-kampaṃ tat-saṃjñaṃ kurvate malāḥ ।।

pitta-pradhānair vātādyaiḥ śaṅkhe śophaḥ sa-śoṇitaiḥ ।
tīvra-dāha-rujā-rāga-pralāpa-jvara-tṛḍ-bhramāḥ ।।

tiktāsyaḥ pīta-vadanaḥ kṣipra-kārī sa śaṅkhakaḥ ।
tri-rātrāj jīvitaṃ hanti sidhyaty apy āśu sādhitaḥ ।।

idhyaty āśu su-sādhitaḥ
pittānubaddhaḥ śaṅkhākṣi-bhrū-lalāṭeṣu mārutaḥ ।
rujaṃ sa-spandanāṃ kuryād anu-sūryodayodayām ।।

ittānubandhaḥ śaṅkhākṣi-
ā-madhyāhnaṃ vivardhiṣṇuḥ kṣud-vataḥ sā viśeṣataḥ ।
a-vyavasthita-śītoṣṇa-sukhā śāmyaty ataḥ param ।।

sūryāvartaḥ sa ity uktā daśa rogāḥ śiro-gatāḥ ।
śirasy eva ca vakṣyante kapāle vyādhayo nava ।।

kapāle pavane duṣṭe garbha-sthasyāpi jāyate ।
sa-varṇo nī-rujaḥ śophas taṃ vidyād upa-śīrṣakam ।।

yathā-doṣodayaṃ brūyāt piṭikārbuda-vidradhīn ।
kapāle kleda-bahulāḥ pittāsṛk-śleṣma-jantubhiḥ ।।

kaṅgu-siddhārthaka-nibhāḥ piṭikāḥ syur arūṃṣikāḥ ।
kaṇḍū-keśa-cyuti-svāpa-raukṣya-kṛt sphuṭanaṃ tvacaḥ ।।

-rūkṣa-kṛt sphuṭanaṃ tvacaḥ
su-sūkṣmaṃ kapha-vātābhyāṃ vidyād dāruṇakaṃ tu tat ।
roma-kūpānugaṃ pittaṃ vātena saha mūrchitam ।।

idyād dāruṇakaṃ ca tat
pracyāvayati romāṇi tataḥ śleṣmā sa-śoṇitaḥ ।
roma-kūpān ruṇaddhy asya tenānyeṣām a-saṃbhavaḥ ।।

tad indra-luptaṃ rujyāṃ ca prāhuś cāceti cāpare ।
khalater api janmaivaṃ śātanaṃ tatra tu kramāt ।।

ad indra-luptaṃ tajjāṃ ca ad indra-luptaṃ tajhjhāṃ ca ad indra-luptaṃ tahnāś ca ad indra-luptaṃ rūḍhyāṃ ca śatanaṃ tatra tu kramāt śadanaṃ tatra tu kramāt 
adanaṃ tatra tu kramāt
sā vātād agni-dagdhābhā pittāt svinna-sirāvṛtā ।
kaphād ghana-tvag varṇāṃś ca yathā-svaṃ nirdiśet tvaci ।।

ittāt snigdha-sirāvṛtā ittāt snigdhā sirāvṛtā ittāt 
pīta-sirāvṛtā
doṣaiḥ sarvākṛtiḥ sarvair a-sādhyā sā nakha-prabhā ।
dagdhāgnineva nī-romā sa-dāhā yā ca jāyate ।।

a-dāhoṣā ca jāyate
śoka-śrama-krodha-kṛtaḥ śarīroṣmā śiro-gataḥ ।
keśān sa-doṣaḥ pacati palitaṃ saṃbhavaty ataḥ ।।

tad vātāt sphuṭitaṃ śyāvaṃ kharaṃ rūkṣaṃ jala-prabham ।
pittāt sa-dāhaṃ pītābhaṃ kaphāt snigdhaṃ vivṛddhi-mat ।।

sthūlaṃ su-śuklaṃ sarvais tu vidyād vyāmiśra-lakṣaṇam ।
śiro-rujodbhavaṃ cānyad vi-varṇaṃ sparśanā-saham ।।

thūlaṃ sa-śuklaṃ sarvais tu
a-sādhyā saṃnipātena khalatiḥ palitāni ca ।
śarīra-pariṇāmotthāny apekṣante rasāyanam ।।

uttarasthāna
śiro-'bhitāpe anila-je vāta-vyādhi-vidhiṃ caret ।
ghṛtam akta-śirā rātrau pibed uṣṇa-payo-'nupaḥ ।।

hṛtam akta-śiro rātrau hṛtābhyakta-śiro rātrau ibet 
sarpiḥ payo-'nupaḥ
māṣān kulatthān mudgān vā tad-vat khāded ghṛtānvitān ।
tailaṃ tilānāṃ kalkaṃ vā kṣīreṇa saha pāyayet ।।

piṇḍopanāha-svedāś ca māṃsa-dhānya-kṛtā hitāḥ ।
vāta-ghna-daśa-mūlādi-siddha-kṣīreṇa secanam ।।

snigdhaṃ nasyaṃ tathā dhūmaḥ śiraḥ-śravaṇa-tarpaṇam ।
varaṇādau gaṇe kṣuṇṇe kṣīram ardhodakaṃ pacet ।।

aruṇādau gaṇe kṣuṇṇe
kṣīrāvaśiṣṭaṃ tac chītaṃ mathitvā sāram āharet ।
tato madhurakaiḥ siddhaṃ nasyaṃ tat pūjitaṃ haviḥ ।।

varge atra pakvaṃ kṣīre ca peyaṃ sarpiḥ sa-śarkaram ।
kārpāsa-majjā tvaṅ mustā sumanaḥ-korakāṇi ca ।।

asmin vipakvaṃ kṣīre ca ārpāsa-majjā tvaṅ mustaṃ 
sumanaḥ-kṣārakāṇi ca
nasyam uṣṇāmbu-piṣṭāni sarva-mūrdha-rujāpaham ।
śarkarā-kuṅkuma-śṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ pittāsṛg-anvaye ।।

pralepaiḥ sa-ghṛtaiḥ kuṣṭha-kuṭilotpala-candanaiḥ ।
vātodreka-bhayād raktaṃ na cāsminn avasecayet ।।

ity a-śāntau cale dāhaḥ kaphe ceṣṭo yathoditaḥ ।
ardhāvabhedake apy eṣā tathā doṣānvayāt kriyā ।।

aphe coṣṇaṃ yathoditam athā-doṣānvayā kriyā 
yathā-doṣānvaye kriyā
śirīṣa-bījāpāmārga-mūlaṃ nasyaṃ viḍānvitam ।
sthirā-raso vā lepe tu prapunnāṭo amla-kalkitaḥ ।।

thirā-raso vā lepo atra
sūryāvarte api tasmiṃs tu sirayāpahared asṛk ।
śiro-'bhitāpe pittotthe snigdhasya vyadhayet sirām ।।

ūryāvarte tu tasmiṃs tu
śītāḥ śiro-mukhālepa-seka-śodhana-vastayaḥ ।
jīvanīya-śṛte kṣīra-sarpiṣī pāna-nasyayoḥ ।।

kartavyaṃ rakta-je apy etat pratyākhyāya ca śaṅkhake ।
śleṣmābhitāpe jīrṇājya-snehitaiḥ kaṭukair vamet ।।

sveda-pralepa-nasyādyā rūkṣa-tīkṣṇoṣṇa-bheṣajaiḥ ।
śasyante copavāso atra nicaye miśram ācaret ।।

śasyate copavāso atra
kṛmi-je śoṇitaṃ nasyaṃ tena mūrchanti jantavaḥ ।
mattāḥ śoṇita-gandhena niryānti ghrāṇa-vaktrayoḥ ।।

iryānti ghrāṇa-vaktrataḥ
su-tīkṣṇa-nasya-dhūmābhyāṃ kuryān nirharaṇaṃ tataḥ ।
viḍaṅga-svarjikā-dantī-hiṅgu-go-mūtra-sādhitam ।।

kaṭu-nimbeṅgudī-pīlu-tailaṃ nasyaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।
ajā-mūtra-drutaṃ nasyaṃ kṛmijit kṛmi-jit param ।।

jā-mūtra-drutaṃ nasye
pūti-matsya-yutaiḥ kuryād dhūmaṃ nāvana-bheṣajaiḥ ।
kṛmibhiḥ pīta-rakta-tvād raktam atra na nirhared ।।
pūti-matsyaḥ kṛmīn hatvā dur-gandha-tvāt tu vāta-je ।।
vātābhitāpa-vihitaḥ kampe dāhād vinā kramaḥ ।
nave janmottaraṃ jāte yojayed upa-śīrṣake ।।

vāta-vyādhi-kriyāṃ pakve karma vidradhi-coditam ।
āma-pakve yathā-yogyaṃ vidradhi-piṭikārbude ।।

arūṃṣikā jalaukobhir hṛtāsrā nimba-vāriṇā ।
siktā prabhūta-lavaṇair limped aśva-śakṛd-rasaiḥ ।।

paṭola-nimba-pattrair vā sa-haridraiḥ su-kalkitaiḥ ।
go-mūtra-jīrṇa-piṇyāka-kṛkavāku-malair api ।।

kapāla-bhṛṣṭaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ vā cūrṇitaṃ taila-saṃyutam ।
rūṃṣikālepanaṃ kaṇḍū-kleda-dāhārti-nāśanam ।।

mālatī-citrakāśvaghna-naktamāla-prasādhitam ।
cācārūṃṣikayos tailam abhyaṅgaḥ kṣura-ghṛṣṭayoḥ ।।

bhyaṅge kṣura-ghṛṣṭayoḥ bhyaṅgaḥ kṣura-mṛṣṭayoḥ
a-śāntau śirasaḥ śuddhyai yateta vamanādibhiḥ ।
vidhyet sirāṃ dāruṇake lālāṭyāṃ śīlayen mṛjām ।।

nāvanaṃ mūrdha-vastiṃ ca lepayec ca sa-mākṣikaiḥ ।
priyāla-bīja-madhuka-kuṣṭha-māṣaiḥ sa-sarṣapaiḥ ।।

āvanaṃ mūrdhni vastiṃ ca
lākṣā-śamyāka-pattraiḍagaja-dhātrī-phalais tathā ।
koradūṣa-tṛṇa-kṣāra-vāri-prakṣālanaṃ hitam ।।

-vāri prakṣālane hitam
indra-lupte yathāsannaṃ sirāṃ viddhvā pralepayet ।
pracchāya gāḍhaṃ kāsīsa-manohvā-tutthakoṣaṇaiḥ ।।

irāṃ viddhvā pralepanam
vanyāmaratarubhyāṃ vā guñjā-mūla-phalais tathā ।
tathā lāṅgalikā-mūlaiḥ karavīra-rasena vā ।।

uṭannaṭa-marubhyāṃ vā hānyāmaratarubhyāṃ vā
sa-kṣaudra-kṣudra-vārtāka-sva-rasena rasena vā ।
dhattūrakasya pattrāṇāṃ bhallātaka-rasena vā ।।

a-kṣaudra-kṣudra-bṛhatī- hallātaka-phalena vā
atha-vā mākṣika-havis-tila-puṣpa-trikaṇṭakaiḥ ।
tailāktā hasti-dantasya maṣī cācauṣadhaṃ param ।।

aṣī vāpy auṣadhaṃ param aṣī vā cauṣadhaṃ param
śukla-romodgame tad-van maṣī meṣa-viṣāṇa-jā ।
varjayed vāriṇā sekaṃ yāvad roma-samudbhavaḥ ।।

āvad roma-samudgamaḥ āvad roma-punar-bhavaḥ
khalatau palite valyāṃ harid-romni ca śodhitam ।
nasya-vaktra-śiro-'bhyaṅga-pradehaiḥ samupācaret ।।

siddhaṃ tailaṃ bṛhaty-ādyair jīvanīyaiś ca nāvanam ।
māsaṃ vā nimba-jaṃ tailaṃ kṣīra-bhuṅ nāvayed yatiḥ ।।

nīlī-śirīṣa-koraṇṭa-bhṛṅga-sva-rasa-bhāvitam ।
śelv-akṣa-tila-rāmāṇāṃ bījaṃ kākāṇḍakī-samam ।।

piṣṭvāja-payasā lohāl liptād arkāṃśu-tāpitāt ।
tailaṃ srutaṃ kṣīra-bhujo nāvanāt palitānta-kṛt ।।

iṣṭvāja-payasā loha- -liptād arkāṃśu-tāpitāt
kṣīrāt sāhacarād bhṛṅgarajasaḥ saurasād rasāt ।
prasthais tailasya kuḍavaḥ siddho yaṣṭī-palānvitaḥ ।।

ṣīrāt sahacarād bhṛṅgaṃ ṣīrāt sāhacarād bhṛṅga- ṃrājataḥ saurasād rasāt 
-rasataḥ saurasād rasāt
nasyaṃ śailāsane bhāṇḍe śṛṅge meṣasya vā sthitaḥ ।
kṣīreṇa ślakṣṇa-piṣṭau vā dugdhikā-karavīrakau ।।

asyaṃ śilā-maye bhāṇḍe asyaṃ śailodbhave bhāṇḍe
utpāṭya palitaṃ deyāv āśaye palitāpahau ।
kṣīraṃ priyālaṃ yaṣṭy-āhvaṃ jīvanīyo gaṇas tilāḥ ।।

kṛṣṇāḥ pralepo vaktrasya harid-roma-valī-hitaḥ ।
tilāḥ sāmalakāḥ padma-kiñjalko madhukaṃ madhu ।।

ari-lopa-valī-hitaḥ
bṛṃhayed rañjayec caitat keśān mūrdha-pralepanāt ।
māṃsī kuṣṭhaṃ tilāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ śārivā nīlam utpalam ।।

ṛṃhayec ca rajec caitat eśān mūrdhnaḥ pralepanāt
kṣaudraṃ ca kṣīra-piṣṭāni keśa-saṃvardhanam param ।
ayo-rajo bhṛṅgarajas tri-phalā kṛṣṇa-mṛttikā ।।

sthitam ikṣu-rase māsaṃ sa-mūlaṃ palitaṃ rajet ।
māṣa-kodrava-dhānyāmlair yavāgūṃs tri-dinoṣitā ।।

ava-kodrava-dhānyāmlair
loha-śuklotkaṭā piṣṭā balākām api rañjayet ।
prapauṇḍarīka-madhuka-pippalī-candanotpalaiḥ ।।

oha-kuṣṭhotkaṭā piṣṭā oha-śuktotkaṭā piṣṭā ohe śuktotkaṭā piṣṭā 
auhe śuklotkaṭā piṣṭā
bhṛṅgarajas-tri-phalotpala-sāri-loha-purīṣa-samanvita-kāri ।
tailam idaṃ paca dāruṇa-hāri luñcita-keśa-ghana-sthira-kāri ।।

-loha-purīṣa-samanvita-dhāri
siddhaṃ dhātrī-rase tailaṃ nasyenābhyañjanena ca ।
sarvān mūrdha-gadān hanti palitāni ca śīlitam ।।

madhūka-yaṣṭī-kṛmijid-viśva-bhṛṅgaiḥ śṛtaṃ haviḥ ।
ṣaḍ-bindu-dānāt tan nasyaṃ sarva-mūrdha-gadāpaham ।।

ṣaḍ-bindu-nāma tan nasyaṃ ṣaḍ-bindu-nāmnā tan nasyaṃ
varī-jīvanti-niryāsa-payobhir yamakaṃ pacet ।
jīvanīyaiś ca tan nasyaṃ sarva-jatrūrdhva-roga-jit ।।

arī-jīvanti-niryāsaiḥ -payobhir yad ghṛtaṃ pacet 
sa-payobhir ghṛtaṃ pacet
mayūraṃ pakṣa-pittāntra-pāda-viṭ-tuṇḍa-varjitam ।
daśa-mūla-balā-rāsnā-madhukais tri-palair yutam ।।

-śakṛt-pāt-tuṇḍa-varjitam -madhukais tri-palaiḥ saham
jale paktvā ghṛta-prasthaṃ tasmin kṣīra-samaṃ pacet ।
kalkitair madhura-dravyaiḥ sarva-jatrūrdhva-roga-jit ।।

tad abhyāsī-kṛtaṃ pāna-vasty-abhyañjana-nāvanaiḥ ।
etenaiva kaṣāyeṇa ghṛta-prasthaṃ vipācayet ।।

catur-guṇena payasā kalkair ebhiś ca kārṣikaiḥ ।
jīvantī-tri-phalā-medā-mṛdvīkarddhi-parūṣakaiḥ ।।

samaṅgā-cavikā-bhārgī-kāśmarī-karkaṭāhvayaiḥ ।
ātmaguptā-mahāmedā-tāla-kharjūra-mastakaiḥ ।।

-tāla-kharjūra-mustakaiḥ
mṛṇāla-bisa-kharjūra-yaṣṭīmadhuka-jīvakaiḥ ।
śatāvarī-vidārīkṣu-bṛhatī-śārivā-yugaiḥ ।।

-bṛhatī-śrāvaṇī-yugaiḥ
mūrvā-śvadaṃṣṭrarṣabhaka-śṛṅgāṭaka-kaserukaiḥ ।
rāsnā-sthirā-tāmalakī-sūkṣmailā-śaṭhi-pauṣkaraiḥ ।।

ūrvā-śvadaṃṣṭraṣabhaka-
punarnavā-tavakṣīrī-kākolī-dhanvayāsakaiḥ ।
madhūkākṣoṭa-vātāma-muñjātābhiṣukair api ।।

adhukākṣoṭa-vātāma-
mahā-māyūram ity etan māyūrād adhikaṃ guṇaiḥ ।
dhātv-indriya-svara-bhraṃśa-śvāsa-kāsārditāpaham ।।

yony-asṛk-śukra-doṣeṣu śastaṃ vandhyā-suta-pradam ।
ākhubhiḥ kukkuṭair haṃsaiḥ śaśaiś ceti prakalpayet ।।

ākhubhiḥ karkaṭair haṃsaiḥ
jatrūrdhva-jānāṃ vyādhīnām eka-triṃśac-chata-dvayam ।
paras-param a-saṃkīrṇaṃ vistareṇa prakāśitam ।।

ka-triṃśaṃ śata-dvayam
ūrdhva-mūlam adhaḥ-śākham ṛṣayaḥ puruṣaṃ viduḥ ।
mūla-prahāriṇas tasmād rogāñ chīghra-taraṃ jayet ।।

sarvendriyāṇi yenāsmin prāṇā yena ca saṃśritāḥ ।
tena tasyottamāṅgasya rakṣāyām ādṛto bhavet ।।

nīlotpalaṃ sotpala-kuṣṭha-yuktaṃ sa-pippalīkaṃ madhukaṃ śatāhvam ।
sa-śṛṅgaveraṃ śirasaḥ pralepaḥ sadyaḥ śiro-roga-vināśanāya ।।

uttarasthāna
vraṇo dvi-dhā nijāgantu-duṣṭa-śuddha-vibhedataḥ ।
nijo doṣaiḥ śarīrotthair āgantur bāhya-hetu-jaḥ ।।

āgantur bāhya-hetubhiḥ
doṣair adhiṣṭhito duṣṭaḥ śuddhas tair an-adhiṣṭhitaḥ ।
saṃvṛta-tvaṃ vivṛta-tā kāṭhinyaṃ mṛdu-tāti vā ।।

āṭhinyaṃ mṛdu-tāpi vā āṭhinyaṃ mṛdu-tāpi ca
aty-utsannāvasanna-tvam aty-auṣṇyam ati-śīta-tā ।
rakta-tvaṃ pāṇḍu-tā kārṣṇyaṃ pūti-pūya-parisrutiḥ ।।

pūti-māṃsa-sirā-snāyu-cchanna-totsaṅgi-tāti-ruk ।
saṃrambha-dāha-śvayathu-kaṇḍv-ādibhir upadrutaḥ ।।

dīrgha-kālānubandhaś ca vidyād duṣṭa-vraṇākṛtim ।
sa pañca-daśa-dhā doṣaiḥ sa-raktais tatra mārutāt ।।

a pañca-dhā pṛthag doṣaiḥ
śyāvaḥ kṛṣṇo aruṇo bhasma-kapotāsthi-nibho api vā ।
mastu-māṃsa-pulākāmbu-tulya-tanv-alpa-saṃsrutiḥ ।।

-kapotāsthi-nibho atha-vā
nir-māṃsas toda-bhedāḍhyo rūkṣaś caṭacaṭāyate ।
pittena kṣipra-jaḥ pīto nīlaḥ kapila-piṅgalaḥ ।।

ittād vahni-prabhaḥ pīto
mūtra-kiṃśuka-bhasmāmbu-tailābhoṣṇa-bahu-srutiḥ ।
kṣārokṣita-kṣata-sama-vyatho rāgoṣma-pāka-vān ।।

kaphena pāṇḍuḥ kaṇḍū-mān bahu-śveta-ghana-srutiḥ ।
sthūlauṣṭhaḥ kaṭhinaḥ snāyu-sirā-jāla-tato alpa-ruk ।।

pravāla-rakto raktena sa-raktaṃ pūyam udgiret ।
vāji-sthāna-samo gandhe yukto liṅgaiś ca paittikaiḥ ।।

a-raktaṃ pūyam īrayet āji-sthāna-samo gandhair 
vāji-sthāna-samo gandho
dvābhyāṃ tribhiś ca sarvaiś ca vidyāl lakṣaṇa-saṃkarāt ।
jihvā-prabho mṛduḥ ślakṣṇaḥ śyāvauṣṭha-piṭikaḥ samaḥ ।।

śyāvauṣṭho a-piṭikaḥ samaḥ
kiñ-cid-unnata-madhyo vā vraṇaḥ śuddho an-upadravaḥ ।
tvag-āmiṣa-sirā-snāyu-saṃdhy-asthīni vraṇāśayāḥ ।।

koṣṭho marma ca tāny aṣṭau duḥ-sādhyāny uttarottaram ।
su-sādhyaḥ sat-tva-māṃsāgni-vayo-bala-vati vraṇaḥ ।।

-vayo-bala-vatāṃ vraṇaḥ
vṛtto dīrghas tri-puṭakaś catur-aśrākṛtiś ca yaḥ ।
tathā sphik-pāyu-meḍhrauṣṭha-pṛṣṭhāntar-vaktra-gaṇḍa-gaḥ ।।

-pṛṣṭhāntar-vaktra-gaṇḍa-jaḥ -pṛṣṭhāntar-vaktra-gaṇḍayoḥ
kṛcchra-sādhyo akṣi-daśana-nāsikāpāṅga-nābhiṣu ।
sevanī-jaṭhara-śrotra-pārśva-kakṣā-staneṣu ca ।।

phena-pūyānila-vahaḥ śalya-vān ūrdhva-nirvamī ।
bhagandaro antar-vadanas tathā kaṭy-asthi-saṃśritaḥ ।।

kuṣṭhināṃ viṣa-juṣṭānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ madhu-mehināṃ ।
vraṇāḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyanti yeṣāṃ ca syur vraṇe vraṇāḥ ।।

eṣāṃ cāpi vraṇe vraṇāḥ
naiva sidhyanti vīsarpa-jvarātīsāra-kāsinām ।
pipāsūnām a-nidrāṇāṃ śvāsinām a-vipākinām ।।

ipāsūnāṃ sa-nidrāṇāṃ
bhinne śiraḥ-kapāle vā mastuluṅgasya darśane ।
snāyu-kledāt sirā-chedād gāmbhīryāt kṛmi-bhakṣaṇāt ।।

asthi-bhedāt sa-śalya-tvāt sa-viṣa-tvād a-tarkitāt ।
mithyā-bandhād ati-snehād raukṣyād romādi-ghaṭṭanāt ।।

kṣobhād a-śuddha-koṣṭha-tvāt sauhityād ati-karśanāt ।
madya-pānād divā-svapnād vyavāyād rātri-jāgarāt ।।

adya-pānād divā-svāpād
vraṇo mithyopacārāc ca naiva sādhyo api sidhyati ।
kapota-varṇa-pratimā yasyāntaḥ kleda-varjitāḥ ।।

aiva sādhyo api rohati
sthirāś cipiṭikā-vanto rohatīti tam ādiśet ।
athātra śophāvasthāyāṃ yathāsannaṃ viśodhanam ।।

thirāś ca piṭikā-vanto
yojyaṃ śopho hi śuddhānāṃ vraṇaś cāśu praśāmyati ।
kuryāc chītopacāraṃ ca śophāvasthasya saṃtatam ।।

uryāc chītopacāraṃ tu
doṣāgnir agni-vat tena prayāti sahasā śamam ।
śophe vraṇe ca kaṭhine vi-varṇe vedanānvite ।।

viṣa-yukte viśeṣeṇa jala-jādyair hared asṛk ।
duṣṭāsre apagate sadyaḥ śopha-rāga-rujāṃ śamaḥ ।।

alaukādyair hared asṛk
hṛte hṛte ca rudhire su-śītaiḥ sparśa-vīryayoḥ ।
su-ślakṣṇais tad-ahaḥ-piṣṭaiḥ kṣīrekṣu-sva-rasa-dravaiḥ ।।

ṣīrekṣu-sva-rasa-drutaiḥ
śata-dhauta-ghṛtopetair muhur anyair a-śoṣibhiḥ ।
pratilomaṃ hito lepaḥ sekābhyaṅgāś ca tat-kṛtāḥ ।।

nyagrodhodumbarāśvattha-plakṣa-vetasa-valkalaiḥ ।
pradeho bhūri-sarpirbhiḥ śopha-nirvāpaṇaḥ param ।।

radeho bhūri-sarpiś ca
vātolbaṇānāṃ stabdhānāṃ kaṭhinānāṃ mahā-rujām ।
srutāsṛjāṃ ca śophānāṃ vraṇānām api cedṛśām ।।

ānūpa-vesavārādyaiḥ svedaḥ somās tilāḥ punaḥ ।
bhṛṣṭā nirvāpitāḥ kṣīre tat-piṣṭā dāha-rug-harāḥ ।।

sthirān manda-rujaḥ śophān snehair vāta-kaphāpahaiḥ ।
abhyajya svedayitvā ca veṇu-nāḍyā śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।।

vimlāpanārthaṃ mṛdnīyāt talenāṅguṣṭhakena vā ।
yava-godhūma-mudgaiś ca siddha-piṣṭaiḥ pralepayet ।।

iddhaiḥ piṣṭaiḥ pralepayet iddhaṃ piṣṭaṃ pralepayet 
ugdha-piṣṭaiḥ pralepayet
vilīyate sa cen naivaṃ tatas tam upanāhayet ।
a-vidagdhas tathā śāntiṃ vidagdhaḥ pākam aśnute ।।

sa-kola-tila-vallomā dadhy-amlā saktu-piṇḍikā ।
sa-kiṇva-kuṣṭha-lavaṇā koṣṇā śastopanāhane ।।

a-kola-tila-vallūra- -dadhy-amlā saktu-piṇḍikā
su-pakve piṇḍite śophe pīḍanair upapīḍite ।
dāraṇaṃ dāraṇārhasya su-kumārasya ceṣyate ।।

guggulv-atasi-go-danta-svarṇakṣīrī-kapota-viṭ ।
kṣārauṣadhāni kṣārāś ca pakva-śopha-vidāraṇam ।।

ṣārauṣadhāni kṣāraś ca
pūya-garbhān aṇu-dvārān sotsaṅgān marma-gān api ।
niḥ-snehaiḥ pīḍana-dravyaiḥ samantāt pratipīḍayet ।।

śuṣyantaṃ samupekṣeta pralepaṃ pīḍanaṃ prati ।
na mukhe cainam ālimpet tathā doṣaḥ prasicyate ।।

kalāya-yava-godhūma-māṣa-mudga-hareṇavaḥ ।
dravyāṇāṃ picchilānāṃ ca tvaṅ-mūlāni prapīḍanam ।।

ravyāṇāṃ picchilānāṃ tu ravyāṇāṃ picchilānāṃ vā
saptasu kṣālanādyeṣu surasāragvadhādikau ।
bhṛśaṃ duṣṭe vraṇe yojyau meha-kuṣṭha-vraṇeṣu ca ।।

atha-vā kṣālanaṃ kvāthaḥ paṭolī-nimba-pattra-jaḥ ।
a-viśuddhe viśuddhe tu nyagrodhādi-tvag-udbhavaḥ ।।

tha-vā kṣālane kvāthaḥ
paṭolī-tila-yaṣṭy-āhva-trivṛd-dantī-niśā-dvayam ।
nimba-pattrāṇi cālepaḥ sa-paṭur vraṇa-śodhanaḥ ।।

a-paṭur vraṇa-śodhanam
vraṇān viśodhayed vartyā sūkṣmāsyān saṃdhi-marma-gān ।
kṛtayā trivṛtā-dantī-lāṅgalī-madhu-saindhavaiḥ ।।

vātābhibhūtān sāsrāvān dhūpayed ugra-vedanān ।
yavājya-bhūrja-madana-śrīveṣṭaka-surāhvayaiḥ ।।

nirvāpayed bhṛśaṃ śītaiḥ pitta-rakta-viṣolbaṇān ।
śuṣkālpa-māṃse gambhīre vraṇa utsādanaṃ hitam ।।

nyagrodha-padmakādibhyām aśvagandhā-balā-tilaiḥ ।
adyān māṃsāda-māṃsāni vidhinopahitāni ca ।।

ihitopahitāni ca idhānopahitāni ca
māṃsaṃ māṃsāda-māṃsena vardhate śuddha-cetasaḥ ।
utsanna-mṛdu-māṃsānāṃ vraṇānām avasādanam ।।

ardhate śuddha-tejasaḥ
jātī-mukula-kāsīsa-manohvāla-purāgnikaiḥ ।
utsanna-māṃsān kaṭhinān kaṇḍū-yuktāṃś cirotthitān ।।

vraṇān su-duḥkha-śodhyāṃś ca śodhayet kṣāra-karmaṇā ।
sravanto aśmarī-jā mūtraṃ ye cānye rakta-vāhinaḥ ।।

raṇān su-duḥkha-sādhyāṃś ca ojayet kṣāra-karmaṇā 
e cānye kṣata-vāhinaḥ
chinnāś ca saṃdhayo yeṣāṃ yathoktair ye ca śodhanaiḥ ।
śodhyamānā na śudhyanti śodhyāḥ syus te agni-karmaṇā ।।

athoktair ye ca sādhanaiḥ ādhyamānā na sidhyanti ādhyāḥ syus te agni-karmaṇā 
ādhyās te cāgni-karmaṇā
śuddhānāṃ ropaṇaṃ yojyam utsādāya yad īritam ।
aśvagandhā ruhā lodhraṃ kaṭphalaṃ madhuyaṣṭikā ।।

śuddhānāṃ ropaṇe yojyam
samaṅgā dhātakī-puṣpaṃ paramaṃ vraṇa-ropaṇam ।
apeta-pūti-māṃsānāṃ māṃsa-sthānām a-rohatām ।।

kalkaṃ saṃrohaṇaṃ kuryāt tilānāṃ madhukānvitam ।
snigdhoṣṇa-tikta-madhura-kaṣāya-tvaiḥ sa sarva-jit ।।

alkaṃ saṃrohaṇe kuryāt alkaḥ saṃrohaṇaṃ kuryāt ilānāṃ madhukānvitaḥ 
-kaṣāyair eṣa sarva-jit
sa kṣaudra-nimba-pattrābhyāṃ yuktaḥ saṃśodhanaṃ param ।
pūrvābhyāṃ sarpiṣā cāsau yuktaḥ syād āśu ropaṇaḥ ।।

uktaḥ saṃśodhanaḥ param uktaḥ syād api ropaṇaḥ
tila-vad yava-kalkaṃ tu ke-cid icchanti tad-vidaḥ ।
sāsra-pitta-viṣāgantu-gambhīrān soṣmaṇo vraṇān ।।

kṣīra-ropaṇa-bhaiṣajya-śṛtenājyena ropayet ।
ropaṇauṣadha-siddhena tailena kapha-vāta-jān ।।

kācchī-lodhrābhayā-sarja-sindūrāñjana-tutthakam ।
cūrṇitaṃ taila-madanair yuktaṃ ropaṇam uttamam ।।

ākṣī-lodhrābhayā-sarja- āṅkṣī-lodhrābhayā-sarja-
samānāṃ sthira-māṃsānāṃ tvak-sthānāṃ cūrṇa iṣyate ।
kakubhodumbarāśvattha-jambū-kaṭphala-lodhra-jaiḥ ।।

vak-sthānāṃ cūrṇam iṣyate
tvak-cūrṇaiś cūrṇitā vraṇāḥ tvak-cūrṇaiś cūrṇitā vraṇāḥ ।
lākṣā-manohvā-mañjiṣṭhā-haritāla-niśā-dvayaiḥ ।।

vacam āśu nigṛhṇāti vak-cūrṇaiś cūrṇito vraṇaḥ
pralepaḥ sa-ghṛta-kṣaudras tvag-viśuddhi-karaḥ param ।
kālīyaka-latāmrāsthi-hema-kālā-rasottamaiḥ ।।

ralepaḥ sa-ghṛta-kṣaudrais
lepaḥ sa-go-maya-rasaḥ sa-varṇa-karaṇaḥ param ।
dagdho vāraṇa-danto antar-dhūmaṃ tailaṃ rasāñjanam ।।

a-varṇa-karaṇo bhavet -dhūmas tailaṃ rasāñjanam
roma-saṃjanano lepas tad-vat taila-pariplutā ।
catuṣ-pān-nakha-romāsthi-tvak-śṛṅga-khura-jā maṣī ।।

vraṇinaḥ śastra-karmoktaṃ pathyā-pathyānnam ādiśet ।
dve pañca-mūle vargaś ca vāta-ghno vātike hitaḥ ।।

raṇināṃ śastra-karmoktaṃ at pathyā-pathyam ādiśet
nyagrodha-padmakādyau tu tad-vat pitta-pradūṣite ।
āragvadhādiḥ śleṣma-ghnaḥ kaphe miśrās tu miśra-je ।।

aphe miśras tu miśra-je aphe miśrās tu miśrake
ebhiḥ prakṣālanaṃ lepo ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ rasa-kriyā ।
cūrṇo vartiś ca saṃyojya vraṇe sapta yathā-yatham ।।

bhiḥ prakṣālanālepa- -ghṛta-taila-rasa-kriyāḥ jātī-nimba-paṭola-pattra-kaṭukā-dārvī-niśā-śārivā- ।।
-mañjiṣṭhābhaya-siktha-tuttha-madhukair naktāhva-bījānvitaiḥ ।।
-mañjiṣṭhābhaya-siktha-tuttha-madhukair naktāhva-bījais tathā sarpiḥ sādhyam anena sūkṣma-vadanā marmāśritāḥ kledino ।।

arpiḥ sādhyam anena sūkṣma-vadanā marmāśritāḥ srāviṇo
arpiḥ siddham anena sūkṣma-vadanā marmāśritāḥ kledino
gambhīrāḥ sa-rujo vraṇāḥ sa-gatayaḥ śudhyanti rohanti ca ।।

ambhīrāḥ sa-rujo vraṇāḥ sa-gatikāḥ śudhyanti rohanti ca
sādhitaṃ sva-rase tailaṃ kākamācyāś catur-guṇe ।
gati-bhājām api hitaṃ vraṇānāṃ ropaṇaṃ param ।।

ati-bhājām api varaṃ

uttarasthāna
sadyo-vraṇā ye sahasā saṃbhavanty abhighātataḥ ।
an-antair api tair aṅgam ucyate juṣṭam aṣṭa-dhā ।।

ghṛṣṭāvakṛtta-vicchinna-pravilambita-pātitam ।
viddhaṃ bhinnaṃ vidalitaṃ tatra ghṛṣṭaṃ lasīkayā ।।

-pravilambi-nipātitam
rakta-leśena vā yuktaṃ sa-ploṣaṃ chedanāt sravet ।
avagāḍhaṃ tataḥ kṛttaṃ vicchinnaṃ syāt tato api ca ।।

pravilambi sa-śeṣe asthni patitaṃ pātitaṃ tanoḥ ।
sūkṣmāsya-śalya-viddhaṃ tu viddhaṃ koṣṭha-vivarjitam ।।

ravilambi sa-śeṣāsthi
bhinnam anyad vidalitaṃ majja-rakta-pariplutam ।
prahāra-pīḍanotpeṣāt sahāsthnā pṛthu-tāṃ gatam ।।

rahāra-pīḍanotpātaiḥ rahāra-pīḍanāt teṣāṃ
sadyaḥ sadyo-vraṇaṃ siñced atha yaṣṭy-āhva-sarpiṣā ।
tīvra-vyathaṃ kavoṣṇena balā-tailena vā punaḥ ।।

kṣatoṣmaṇo nigrahārthaṃ tat-kālaṃ visṛtasya ca ।
kaṣāya-śīta-madhura-snigdhā lepādayo hitāḥ ।।

sadyo-vraṇeṣv āyateṣu saṃdhānārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
madhu-sarpiś ca yuñjīta pitta-ghnīś ca himāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

adhu-sarpiḥ prayuñjīta
sa-saṃrambheṣu kartavyam ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca śodhanam ।
upavāso hitaṃ bhuktaṃ pratataṃ rakta-mokṣaṇam ।।

pavāso hitas tatra
ghṛṣṭe vidalite caiṣa su-tarām iṣyate vidhiḥ ।
tayor hy alpaṃ sravaty asraṃ pākas tenāśu jāyate ।।

aty-artham asraṃ sravati prāya-śo anya-tra vikṣate ।
tato rakta-kṣayād vāyau kupite ati-rujā-kare ।।

ty-artham asraṃ vamati rāya-śo anya-tra ca kṣate
sneha-pāna-parīṣeka-sveda-lepopanāhanam ।
sneha-vastiṃ ca kurvīta vāta-ghnauṣadha-sādhitam ।।

nehair vastiṃ ca kurvīta āta-ghnauṣadha-sādhitaiḥ
iti sāptāhikaḥ proktaḥ sadyo-vraṇa-hito vidhiḥ ।
saptāhād gata-vege tu pūrvoktaṃ vidhim ācaret ।।

ti saptāhikaḥ proktaḥ
prāyaḥ sāmānya-karmedaṃ vakṣyate tu pṛthak pṛthak ।
ghṛṣṭe rujaṃ nigṛhyāśu vraṇe cūrṇāni yojayet ।।

kalkādīny avakṛtte tu vicchinna-pravilambinoḥ ।
sīvanaṃ vidhinoktena bandhanaṃ cānu pīḍanam ।।

andhanaṃ cāśu pīḍanam
a-sādhyaṃ sphuṭitaṃ netram a-dīrṇaṃ lambate tu yat ।
saṃniveśya yathā-sthānam a-vyāviddha-siraṃ bhiṣak ।।

dīrṇaṃ lambate tu yat aṃniveśya yathā-sthānaṃ 
sūcyā vidhyet sirāṃ bhiṣak
pīḍayet pāṇinā padma-palāśāntaritena tat ।
tato asya secane nasye tarpaṇe ca hitaṃ haviḥ ।।

arpaṇe kathitaṃ haviḥ
vipakvam ājaṃ yaṣṭy-āhva-jīvakarṣabhakotpalaiḥ ।
sa-payaskaiḥ paraṃ tad dhi sarva-netrābhighāta-jit ।।

gala-pīḍāvasanne akṣṇi vamanotkāsana-kṣavāḥ ।
prāṇāyāmo atha-vā kāryaḥ kriyā ca kṣata-netra-vat ।।

ala-pīḍo avasanne akṣṇi amanotkleśana-kṣavāḥ
karṇe sthānāc cyute syūte śrotas tailena pūrayet ।
kṛkāṭikāyāṃ chinnāyāṃ nirgacchaty api mārute ।।

arṇe sthāna-cyute syūte rotas tailena pūrayet
samaṃ niveśya badhnīyāt syūtvā śīghraṃ nir-antaram ।
ājena sarpiṣā cātra pariṣekaḥ praśasyate ।।

amāṃ niveśya badhnīyāt ājena sarpiṣā tatra
uttāno annāni bhuñjīta śayīta ca su-yantritaḥ ।
ghātaṃ śākhāsu tiryak-sthaṃ gātre samyaṅ-niveśite ।।

syūtvā vellita-bandhena badhnīyād ghana-vāsasā ।
carmaṇā goṣ-phaṇā-bandhaḥ kāryaś cā-saṃgate vraṇe ।।

āryaś cāṃsa-gate vraṇe āryaś cāṃśa-gate vraṇe
pādau vilambi-muṣkasya prokṣya netre ca vāriṇā ।
praveśya vṛṣaṇau sīvyet sevanyā tunna-saṃjñayā ।।

evanyā picu-yuktayā īvanyā picu-yuktayā
kāryaś ca goṣ-phaṇā-bandhaḥ kaṭyām āveśya paṭṭakam ।
sneha-sekaṃ na kurvīta tatra klidyati hi vraṇaḥ ।।

atra klidyanti hi vraṇāḥ ena klidyanti hi vraṇāḥ
kālānusāry-agurv-elā-jātī-candana-parpaṭaiḥ ।
śilā-dārvy-amṛtā-tutthaiḥ siddhaṃ tailaṃ ca ropaṇam ।।

-jātī-candana-padmakaiḥ
chinnāṃ niḥśeṣataḥ śākhāṃ dagdhvā tailena yuktitaḥ ।
badhnīyāt kośa-bandhena tato vraṇa-vad ācaret ।।

agdhvā tailena yuktibhiḥ
kāryā śalyāhṛte viddhe bhaṅgād vidalite kriyā ।
śiraso apahṛte śalye vāla-vartiṃ praveśayet ।।

mastuluṅga-sruteḥ kruddho hanyād enaṃ calo anya-thā ।
vraṇe rohati caikaikaṃ śanair apanayet kacam ।।

astuluṅga-srute kruddho
mastuluṅga-srutau khāden mastiṣkān anya-jīva-jān ।
śalye hṛte aṅgād anyasmāt sneha-vartiṃ nidhāpayet ।।

dūrāvagāḍhāḥ sūkṣmāsyā ye vraṇāḥ sruta-śoṇitāḥ ।
secayec cakra-tailena sūkṣma-netrārpitena tān ।।

bhinne koṣṭhe asṛjā pūrṇe mūrchā-hṛt-pārśva-vedanāḥ ।
jvaro dāhas tṛḍ ādhmānaṃ bhaktasyān-abhinandanam ।।

saṅgo viṇ-mūtra-marutāṃ śvāsaḥ svedo akṣi-rakta-tā ।
loha-gandhi-tvam āsyasya syād gātre ca vi-gandha-tā ।।

āmāśaya-sthe rudhire rudhiraṃ chardayaty api ।
ādhmānenāti-mātreṇa śūlena ca viśasyate ।।

śūlena ca vinaśyati śūlena ca viśiṣyate
pakvāśaya-sthe rudhire sa-śūlaṃ gauravaṃ bhavet ।
nābher adhas-tāc chīta-tvaṃ khebhyo raktasya cāgamaḥ ।।

a-bhinno apy āśayaḥ sūkṣmaiḥ srotobhir abhipūryate ।
asṛjā syandamānena pārśve mūtreṇa vasti-vat ।।

tatrāntar-lohitaṃ śīta-pādocchvāsa-karānanam ।
raktākṣaṃ pāṇdu-vadanam ānaddhaṃ ca vivarjayet ।।

āmāśaya-sthe vamanaṃ hitaṃ pakvāśayāśrite ।
virecanaṃ nirūhaṃ ca niḥ-snehoṣṇair viśodhanaiḥ ।।

itaṃ pakvāśayāśraye itaṃ pakvāśaya-sthite 
niḥ-snehoṣṇair viśodhanam
yava-kola-kulatthānāṃ rasaiḥ sneha-vivarjitaiḥ ।
bhuñjītānnaṃ yavāgūṃ vā pibet saindhava-saṃyutām ।।

ibet saindhava-saṃyutam
ati-niḥsruta-raktas tu bhinna-koṣṭhaḥ pibed asṛk ।
kliṣṭa-cchinnāntra-bhedena koṣṭha-bhedo dvi-dhā smṛtaḥ ।।

ti-niḥsṛta-raktas tu linna-bhinnāntra-bhedena 
śliṣṭa-cchinnāntra-bhedena
mūrchādayo alpāḥ prathame dvitīye tv ati-bādhakāḥ ।
kliṣṭāntraḥ saṃśayī dehī chinnāntro naiva jīvati ।।

linnāntraḥ saṃśayī dehī liṣṭāntraḥ saṃśaye dehī śliṣṭāntraḥ saṃśayī dehī 
hinnāntro naiva jīvati
yathā-svaṃ mārgam āpannā yasya viṇ-mūtra-mārutāḥ ।
vy-upadravaḥ sa bhinne api koṣṭhe jīvaty a-saṃśayam ।।

a-bhinnam antraṃ niṣkrāntaṃ praveśyaṃ na tv ato anya-thā ।
utpaṅgila-śiro-grastaṃ tad apy eke vadanti tu ।।

rogala-śiro-grastaṃ roṅgila-śiro-grastaṃ upuṅgala-śiro-grastaṃ 
ayaṅgila-śiro-grastaṃ
prakṣālya payasā digdhaṃ tṛṇa-śoṇita-pāṃsubhiḥ ।
praveśayet kḷpta-nakho ghṛtenāktaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।।

kṣīreṇārdrī-kṛtaṃ śuṣkaṃ bhūri-sarpiḥ-pariplutam ।
aṅgulyā pramṛśet kaṇṭhaṃ jalenodvejayed api ।।

tathāntrāṇi viśanty antas tat-kālaṃ pīḍayanti ca ।
vraṇa-saukṣmyād bahu-tvād vā koṣṭham antram an-āviśat ।।

at-kālaṃ pīḍayeta ca
tat-pramāṇena jaṭharaṃ pāṭayitvā praveśayet ।
yathā-sthānaṃ sthite samyak antre sīvyed anu vraṇam ।।

athā-sthāna-sthite samyag
sthānād apetam ādatte jīvitaṃ kupitaṃ ca tat ।
veṣṭayitvānu paṭṭena ghṛtena pariṣecayet ।।

īvitaṃ kupitaṃ ca yat
cūrṇair yathoktaiḥ saṃdhānaṃ kṛtvā kṣaudra-ghṛta-plutaiḥ ।
tataḥ kavalikāṃ dattvā veṣṭayed anu-pūrva-śaḥ ।।

pāyayeta tataḥ koṣṇaṃ citrā-taila-yutaṃ payaḥ ।
mṛdu-kriyārthaṃ śakṛto vāyoś cādhaḥ-pravṛttaye ।।

āyayet taṃ tataḥ koṣṇaṃ itra-taila-yutaṃ payaḥ
anuvarteta varṣaṃ ca yathoktaṃ vraṇa-yantraṇām ।
udarān medaso vartiṃ nirgatāṃ bhasmanā mṛdā ।।

athoktaṃ vraṇa-yantraṇam
avakīrya kaṣāyair vā ślakṣṇair mūlais tataḥ samam ।
dṛḍhaṃ baddhvā ca sūtreṇa vardhayet kuśalo bhiṣak ।।

ślakṣṇair mūle tataḥ samam ślakṣṇaiś cūrṇais tataḥ samam
tīkṣṇenāgni-prataptena śastreṇa sakṛd eva tu ।
syād anya-thā rug āṭopo mṛtyur vā chidyamānayā ।।

sa-kṣaudre ca vraṇe baddhe su-jīrṇe anne ghṛtaṃ pibet ।
kṣīraṃ vā śarkarā-citrā-lākṣā-gokṣurakaiḥ śṛtam ।।

a-kṣaudre tu vraṇe baddhe u-jīrṇānno ghṛtaṃ pibet
rug-dāha-jit sa-yaṣṭy-āhvaiḥ paraṃ pūrvodito vidhiḥ ।
medo-granthy-uditaṃ tatra tailam abhyañjane hitam ।।

edo-granthy-uditaṃ cātra
tālīśaṃ padmakaṃ māṃsī hareṇv-aguru-candanam ।
haridre padma-bījāni sośīraṃ madhukaṃ ca taiḥ ।।

pakvaṃ sadyo-vraṇeṣūktaṃ tailaṃ ropaṇam uttamam ।
gūḍha-prahārābhihate patite viṣamoccakaiḥ ।।

ūḍha-prahārābhihate
kāryaṃ vātāsra-jit tṛpti-mardanābhyañjanādikam ।
viśliṣṭa-dehaṃ mathitaṃ kṣīṇaṃ marmāhataṃ hatam ।।

uryād vātāsṛg-uktaṃ hi -mardanābhyaṅga-śodhanam 
mardanābhyaṅga-śodhanam
ṣīṇaṃ marmāhatāhatam ṣīṇaṃ marmāhataṃ ca tam
vāsayet taila-pūrṇāyāṃ droṇyāṃ māṃsa-rasāśinam ।।

uttarasthāna
pāta-ghātādibhir dve-dhā bhaṅgo asthnāṃ saṃdhy-a-saṃdhitaḥ ।
prasāraṇākuñcanayor a-śaktiḥ saṃdhi-mukta-tā ।।

haṅgo asthnaḥ saṃdhy-a-saṃdhi-gaḥ haṅgo asthnaḥ 
saṃdhy-a-saṃdhitaḥ
itarasmin bhṛśaṃ śophaḥ sarvāvasthāsv ati-vyathā ।
a-śaktiś ceṣṭite alpe api pīḍyamāne sa-śabda-tā ।।

arvāvasthāsv ati-vyathaḥ
samāsād iti bhaṅgasya lakṣaṇaṃ bahu-dhā tu tat ।
bhidyate bhaṅga-bhedena tasya sarvasya sādhanam ।।

yathā syād upayogāya tathā tad upadekṣyate ।
prājyāṇu-dāri yat tv asthi sparśe śabdaṃ karoti yat ।।

rājyāṇu-dāri yac cāsthi
yatrāsthi-leśaḥ praviśen madhyam asthno vidāritaḥ ।
bhagnaṃ yac cābhighātena kiñ-cid evāvaśeṣitam ।।

hagnaṃ yad abhighātena hagnaṃ yad vābhighātena
unnamyamānaṃ kṣata-vad yac ca majjani majjati ।
tad duḥ-sādhyaṃ kṛśā-śakta-vātalālpāśinām api ।।

bhinnaṃ kapālaṃ yat kaṭyāṃ saṃdhi-muktaṃ cyutaṃ ca yat ।
jaghanaṃ prati piṣṭaṃ ca bhagnaṃ yat tad vivarjayet ।।

hinnaṃ kapālaṃ yat kaṭyāḥ
a-saṃśliṣṭa-kapālaṃ ca lalāṭaṃ cūrṇitaṃ tathā ।
yac ca bhagnaṃ bhavec chaṅkha-śiraḥ-pṛṣṭha-stanāntare ।।

samyag-yamitam apy asthi dur-nyāsād dur-nibandhanāt ।
saṃkṣobhād api yad gacched vi-kriyāṃ tad vivarjayet ।।

i-kriyāṃ tac ca varjayet
ādito yac ca dur-jātam asthi saṃdhir athāpi vā ।
taruṇāsthīni bhujyante bhajyante nalakāni tu ।।

aruṇāsthīni namyante hajyante nalakāni ca
kapālāni vibhidyante sphuṭanty anyāni bhūyasā ।
athāvanatam unnamyam unnataṃ cāvapīḍayet ।।

apālāsthīni bhidyante
āñched atikṣiptam adho-gataṃ copari vartayet ।
āñchanotpīḍanonnāma-carma-saṃkṣepa-bandhanaiḥ ।।

āñched a-vikṣiptam adho-
saṃdhīñ charīra-gān sarvāṃś calān apy a-calān api ।
ity etaiḥ sthāpanopāyaiḥ samyak saṃsthāpya niś-calam ।।

amyak saṃsthāpya niś-calān
paṭṭaiḥ prabhūta-sarpirbhiḥ veṣṭayitvā sukhais tataḥ ।
kadambodumbarāśvattha-sarjārjuna-palāśa-jaiḥ ।।

vaṃśodbhavair vā pṛthubhis tanubhiḥ su-niveśitaiḥ ।
su-ślakṣṇaiḥ sa-pratistambhair valkalaiḥ śakalair api ।।

u-ślakṣṇaiḥ sa-pratistambhair
kuśāhvayaiḥ samaṃ bandhaṃ paṭṭasyopari yojayet ।
śithilena hi bandhena saṃdhi-sthairyaṃ na jāyate ।।

aṃdheḥ sthairyaṃ na jāyate
gāḍhenāti rujā-dāha-pāka-śvayathu-saṃbhavaḥ ।
try-ahāt try-ahād ṛtau gharme saptāhān mokṣayed dhime ।।

āḍhenāpi rujā-dāha-
sādhāraṇe tu pañcāhād bhaṅga-doṣa-vaśena vā ।
nyagrodhādi-kaṣāyeṇa tataḥ śītena secayet ।।

hagna-doṣa-vaśena vā haṅge doṣa-vaśena vā
taṃ pañca-mūla-pakvena payasā tu sa-vedanam ।
sukhoṣṇaṃ vāvacāryaṃ syāc cakra-tailaṃ vijānatā ।।

añca-mūla-vipakvena c sukhoṣṇam avacāryaṃ syāc
vibhajya deśaṃ kālaṃ ca vāta-ghnauṣadha-saṃyutam ।
pratataṃ seka-lepāṃś ca vidadhyād bhṛśa-śītalān ।।

ibhajya deśa-kālau ca āta-ghnauṣadha-sādhitam
gṛṣṭi-kṣīraṃ sa-sarpiṣkaṃ madhurauṣadha-sādhitam ।
prātaḥ prātaḥ pibed bhagnaḥ śītalaṃ lākṣayā yutam ।।

sa-vraṇasya tu bhagnasya vraṇo madhu-ghṛtottaraiḥ ।
kaṣāyaiḥ pratisāryo atha śeṣo bhaṅgoditaḥ kramaḥ ।।

aṣāyaiḥ pratisāryo vā
lambāni vraṇa-māṃsāni pralipya madhu-sarpiṣā ।
saṃdadhīta vraṇān vaidyo bandhanaiś copapādayet ।।

tān samān su-sthitāñ jñātvā phalinī-lodhra-kaṭphalaiḥ ।
samaṅgā-dhātakī-yuktaiś cūrṇitair avacūrṇayet ।।

dhātakī-lodhra-cūrṇair vā rohanty āśu tathā vraṇāḥ ।
iti bhaṅga upakrāntaḥ sthira-dhātor ṛtau hime ।।

māṃsalasyālpa-doṣasya su-sādhyo dāruṇo anya-thā ।
pūrva-madhyānta-vayasām eka-dvi-tri-guṇaiḥ kramāt ।।

u-sādho dāruṇo anya-thā
māsaiḥ sthairyaṃ bhavet saṃdher yathoktaṃ bhajatāṃ vidhim ।
kaṭī-jaṅghoru-bhagnānāṃ kapāṭa-śayanaṃ hitam ।।

athoktaṃ bhajato vidhim
yantraṇārthaṃ tathā kīlāḥ pañca kāryā nibandhanāḥ ।
jaṅghorvoḥ pārśvayor dvau dvau tala ekaś ca kīlakaḥ ।।

śroṇyāṃ vā pṛṣṭha-vaṃśe vā vakṣasy akṣakayos tathā ।
vimokṣe bhagna-saṃdhīnāṃ vidhim evaṃ samācaret ।।

akṣasy aṃśakayos tathā aktrasyākṣakayos tathā 
vidhim enaṃ samācaret
saṃdhīṃś cira-vimuktāṃs tu snigdha-svinnān mṛdū-kṛtān ।
uktair vidhānair buddhyā ca yathā-svaṃ sthānam ānayet ।।

aṃdhīṃś cira-vimuktāṃś ca ktair vidhānair yuktyā ca 
ktair vidhānair yuktyā vā
a-saṃdhi-bhagne rūḍhe tu viṣamolbaṇa-sādhite ।
āpothya bhaṅgaṃ yamayet tato bhagna-vad ācaret ।।

-saṃdhi-bhagne rūḍhe ca iṣamolbaṇa-sādhanaiḥ
bhagnaṃ naiti yathā pākaṃ prayateta tathā bhiṣak ।
pakva-māṃsa-sirā-snāyuḥ saṃdhiḥ śleṣaṃ na gacchati ।।

haṅgo naiti yathā pākaṃ
vāta-vyādhi-vinirdiṣṭān snehān bhagnasya yojayet ।
catuṣ-prayogān balyāṃś ca vasti-karma ca śīlayet ।।

śāly-ājya-rasa-dugdhādyaiḥ pauṣṭikair a-vidāhibhiḥ ।
mātrayopacared bhagnaṃ saṃdhi-saṃśleṣa-kāribhiḥ ।।
glānir na śasyate tasya saṃdhi-viśleṣa-kṛd dhi sā ।।lavaṇaṃ kaṭukaṃ kṣāram amlaṃ maithunam ātapam ।।vyāyāmaṃ ca na seveta bhagno rūkṣaṃ ca bhojanam ।।
kṛṣṇāṃs tilān vi-rajaso dṛḍha-vastra-baddhān sapta kṣapā vahati vāriṇi vāsayet ।
saṃśoṣayed anu-dinaṃ pravisārya caitān kṣīre tathaiva madhuka-kvathite ca toye ।।

aṃśoṣayed anu-dinaṃ pratisārya caitān aṃśoṣayed anu-dinaṃ 
pravibhāvya caitān
punar api pīta-payaskāṃs tān pūrva-vad eva śoṣitān bāḍham ।
vigata-tuṣān a-rajaskān saṃcūrṇya su-cūrṇitair yuñjyāt ।।

aṃcūrṇya vicūrṇitair yuñjyāt
nalada-vālaka-lohitayaṣṭikā-nakha-miśi-plava-kuṣṭha-balā-trayaiḥ ।
aguru-kuṅkuma-candana-śārivā-sarala-sarja-rasāmaradārubhiḥ ।।

padmakādi-gaṇopetais tila-piṣṭaṃ tataś ca tat ।
samasta-gandha-bhaiṣajya-siddha-dugdhena pīḍayet ।।

ila-piṣṭaṃ tataś ca tam
śaileya-rāsnāṃśumatī-kaseru-kālānusārī-nata-pattra-lodhraiḥ ।
sa-kṣīraśuklaiḥ sa-payaḥ sa-dūrvais tailaṃ pacet tan naladādibhiś ca ।।

vak-kṣīra-yuktaiḥ payasā sa-dūrvais a-kṣīra-yuktais payasā sa-dūrvais 
a-kṣīra-yuktais sa-payaḥ sa-dūrvais
gandha-tailam idam uttamam asthi-sthairya-kṛj jayati cāśu vikārān ।
vāta-pitta-janitān ati-vīryān vyāpino api vividhair upayogaiḥ ।।

āta-pitta-janitān ati-vīryaṃ āta-pitta-janitān ati-vīrya- -vyāpino api vividhair upayogaiḥ

uttarasthāna
hasty-aśva-pṛṣṭha-gamana-kaṭhinotkaṭakāsanaiḥ ।
arśo-nidānābhihitair aparaiś ca niṣevitaiḥ ।।

-kaṭhinotkaṭukāsanaiḥ
an-iṣṭā-dṛṣṭa-pākena sadyo vā sādhu-garhaṇaiḥ ।
prāyeṇa piṭikā-pūrvo yo aṅgule dvy-aṅgule api vā ।।

n-iṣṭa-diṣṭa-pākena
pāyor vraṇo antar bāhyo vā duṣṭāsṛṅ-māṃsa-go bhavet ।
vasti-mūtrāśayābhyāsa-gata-tvāt syandanātmakaḥ ।।

āyau vraṇo antar bāhyo vā
bhagandaraḥ sa sarvāṃś ca dārayaty a-kriyā-vataḥ ।
bhaga-vasti-gudāṃs teṣu dīryamāṇeṣu bhūribhiḥ ।।

hagandaraḥ sa sarvaś ca hagandaraḥ sa sarvasya
vāta-mūtra-śakṛc-chukraṃ khaiḥ sūkṣmair vamati kramāt ।
doṣaiḥ pṛthag yutaiḥ sarvair āgantuḥ so aṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

āgantuś cāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ
a-pakvaṃ piṭikāṃ āhuḥ pāka-prāptaṃ bhagandaram ।
gūḍha-mūlāṃ sa-saṃrambhāṃ rug-āḍhyāṃ rūḍha-kopinīm ।।

bhagandara-karīṃ vidyāt piṭikāṃ na tv ato anya-thā ।
tatra śyāvāruṇā toda-bheda-sphuraṇa-ruk-karī ।।

piṭikā mārutāt pittād uṣṭra-grīvā-vad ucchritā ।
rāgiṇī tanur ūṣmāḍhyā jvara-dhūmāyanānvitā ।।

āgiṇī tanu-sūkṣmā ca
sthirā snigdhā mahā-mūlā pāṇḍuḥ kaṇḍū-matī kaphāt ।
śyāvā tāmrā sa-dāhoṣā ghora-rug vāta-pitta-jā ।।

śyāva-tāmrā sa-dāhoṣā
pāṇḍurā kiñ-cid-ā-śyāvā kṛcchra-pākā kaphānilāt ।
pādāṅguṣṭha-samā sarvair doṣair nānā-vidha-vyathā ।।

śūlā-rocaka-tṛḍ-dāha-jvara-cchardir-upadrutā ।
vraṇa-tāṃ yānti tāḥ pakvāḥ pramādāt tatra vāta-jā ।।

cīyate aṇu-mukhaiś chidraiḥ śata-ponaka-vat kramāt ।
acchaṃ sravadbhir āsrāvam ajasraṃ phena-saṃyutam ।।

īryate aṇu-mukhaiś chidraiḥ śata-ponaka-vaktra-vat
śata-ponaka-saṃjño ayam uṣṭra-grīvas tu pitta-jaḥ ।
bahu-picchā-parisrāvī parisrāvī kaphodbhavaḥ ।।

vāta-pittāj parikṣepī parikṣipya gudaṃ gatiḥ ।
jāyate paritas tatra prākāraṃ parikheva ca ।।

rākāra-parikheva ca
ṛjur vāta-kaphād ṛjvyā gudo gatyātra dīryate ।
kapha-pitte tu pūrvotthaṃ dur-nāmāśritya kupyataḥ ।।

udo gatyā tu dīryate udo gatyā nu dīryate 
kapha-pitte tu pūrvoktaṃ
arśo-mūle tataḥ śophaḥ kaṇḍū-dāhādi-mān bhavet ।
sa śīghraṃ pakva-bhinno asya kledayan mūlam arśasaḥ ।।

sravaty ajasraṃ gatibhir ayam arśo-bhagandaraḥ ।
sarva-jaḥ śambukāvartaḥ śambūkāvarta-saṃnibhaḥ ।।

gatayo dārayanty asmin rug-vegair dāruṇair gudam ।
asthi-leśo abhyavahṛto māṃsa-gṛddhyā yadā gudam ।।

kṣiṇoti tiryaṅ nirgacchann un-mārgaṃ kṣatato gatiḥ ।
syāt tataḥ pūya-dīrṇāyāṃ māṃsa-kothena tatra ca ।।

ṣaṇoti tiryaṅ nirgacchan yāt tadā pūya-dīrṇāyāṃ
jāyante kṛmayas tasya khādantaḥ parito gudam ।
vidārayanti na cirād un-mārgī kṣata-jaś ca saḥ ।।

āyante kṛmayas tebhyaḥ n-mārgī kṣata-jas tu saḥ
teṣu rug-dāha-kaṇḍv-ādīn vidyād vraṇa-niṣedhataḥ ।
ṣaṭ kṛcchra-sādhanās teṣāṃ nicaya-kṣata-jau tyajet ।।

idyād vraṇa-vibhaktitaḥ
pravāhiṇīṃ valīṃ prāptaṃ sevanīṃ vā samāśritam ।
athāsya piṭikām eva tathā yatnād upācaret ।।

śuddhy-asṛk-sruti-sekādyair yathā pākaṃ na gacchati ।
pāke punar upasnigdhaṃ sveditaṃ cāvagāhataḥ ।।

yantrayitvārśasam iva paśyet samyag bhagandaram ।
arvācīnaṃ parācīnam antar-mukha-bahir-mukham ।।

vācīnaṃ parācīnam
athāntar-mukham eṣitvā samyak śastreṇa pāṭayet ।
bahir-mukhaṃ ca niḥśeṣaṃ tataḥ kṣāreṇa sādhayet ।।

agninā vā bhiṣak sādhu kṣāreṇaivoṣṭra-kandharam ।
nāḍīr ekāntarāḥ kṛtvā pāṭayec chata-ponakam ।।

āḍīm ekāntaraṃ kṛtvā āṭayec chata-ponake
tāsu rūḍhāsu śeṣāś ca mṛtyur dīrṇe gude anya-thā ।
parikṣepiṇi cāpy evaṃ nāḍy-uktaiḥ kṣāra-sūtrakaiḥ ।।

arśo-bhagandare pūrvam arśāṃsi pratisādhayet ।
tyaktvopacaryaḥ kṣata-jaḥ śalyaṃ śalya-vatas tataḥ ।।

rśāṃsi pratisārayet
āharec ca tathā dadyāt kṛmi-ghnaṃ lepa-bhojanam ।
piṇḍa-nāḍy-ādayaḥ svedāḥ su-snigdhā ruji pūjitāḥ ।।

āhareta tathā dadyāt āharet tat tathā dadyāt āharet 
tu tathā dadyāt
sarva-tra ca bahu-cchidre chedān ālocya yojayet ।
go-tīrtha-sarvato-bhadra-dala-lāṅgala-lāṅgalān ।।

arva-trāpi bahu-cchidre
pārśvaṃ gatena śastreṇa cchedo go-tīrthako mataḥ ।
sarvataḥ sarvato-bhadraḥ pārśva-cchedo ardha-lāṅgalaḥ ।।

ārśva-gatena śastreṇa ārśvāgatena śastreṇa
pārśva-dvaye lāṅgalakaḥ samastāṃś cāgninā dahet ।
āsrāva-mārgān niḥśeṣaṃ naivaṃ vikurute punaḥ ।।

āsrāva-mārgān niḥśeṣān
yateta koṣṭha-śuddhau ca bhiṣak tasyāntarāntarā ।
lepo vraṇe biḍālāsthi tri-phalā-rasa-kalkitam ।।

ateta koṣṭha-śuddhyai ca ateta koṣṭha-saṃśuddhau 
ri-phalā-rasa-kalkitaḥ
jyotiṣmatī-malayu-lāṅgali-śelu-pāṭhā-kumbhāgni-sarja-karavīra-vacā-sudhārkaiḥ ।
abhyañjanāya vipaceta bhagandarāṇāṃ tailaṃ vadanti paramaṃ hitam etad eṣām ।।

-kumbhāgni-sarji-karavīra-vacā-sudhārkaiḥ 
ailaṃ vadanti paramaṃ hitam etad eva
madhuka-lodhra-kaṇā-truṭi-reṇukā-dvi-rajanī-phalinī-paṭu-śārivāḥ ।
kamala-kesara-padmaka-dhātakī-madana-sarja-rasāmaya-rodikāḥ ।।

-madana-sarja-rasāmaya-lodhrakāḥ
sa-bījapūra-cchadanair ebhis tailaṃ vipācitam ।
bhagandarāpacī-kuṣṭha-madhu-meha-vraṇāpaham ।।

madhu-taila-yutā viḍaṅga-sāra-tri-phalā-māgadhikā-kaṇāś ca līḍhāḥ ।
kṛmi-kuṣṭha-bhagandara-prameha-kṣata-nāḍī-vraṇa-ropaṇā bhavanti ।।

-tri-phalā-māgadhikoṣaṇāś ca līḍhāḥ 
-kṣata-nāḍī-vraṇa-rohaṇā bhavanti
amṛtā-truṭi-vella-vatsakaṃ kali-pathyāmalakāni gugguluḥ ।
krama-vṛddham idaṃ madhu-drutaṃ piṭikā-sthaulya-bhagandarāñ jayet ।।

rama-vṛddham idaṃ madhu-plutaṃ
māgadhikāgni-kaliṅga-viḍaṅgair bilva-ghṛtaiḥ sa-varā-pala-ṣaṭkaiḥ ।
guggulunā sadṛśena sametaiḥ kṣaudra-yutaiḥ sakalāmaya-nāśaḥ ।।

āgadhikāgni-kaliṅga-viḍaṅgais ulya-ghṛtaiḥ 
sa-varā-pala-ṣaṭkaiḥ
guggulu-pañca-palaṃ palikāṃśā māgadhikā tri-phalā ca pṛthak syāt ।
tvak-truṭi-karṣa-yutaṃ madhu-līḍhaṃ kuṣṭha-bhagandara-gulma-gati-ghnam ।।

śṛṅgavera-rajo-yuktaṃ tad eva ca su-bhāvitam ।
kvāthena daśa-mūlasya viśeṣād vāta-roga-jit ।।

uttamā-khadira-sāra-jaṃ rajaḥ śīlayann asana-vāri-bhāvitam ।
