hanti tulya-mahiṣākṣa-mākṣikaṃ kuṣṭha-meha-piṭikā-bhagandarān ।।

śīlayed anala-vāri-bhāvitam śīlayed asana-vāri-bhāvitam 
anti tulya-mahiṣākhya-mākṣikaṃ
bhagandareṣv eṣa viśeṣa uktaḥ śeṣāṇi tu vyañjana-sādhanāni ।
vraṇādhikārāt pariśīlanāc ca samyag viditvaupayikaṃ vidadhyāt ।।

amyag viditvauṣadhikaṃ vidadhyāt
aśva-pṛṣṭha-gamanaṃ cala-rodhaṃ madya-maithunam a-jīrṇam a-sātmyam ।
sāhasāni vividhāni ca rūḍhe vatsaraṃ parihared adhikaṃ vā ।।

atsaraṃ parihared adhikaṃ ca

uttarasthāna
kapha-pradhānāḥ kurvanti medo-māṃsāsra-gā malāḥ ।
vṛttonnataṃ yaṃ śvayathuṃ sa granthir grathanāt smṛtaḥ ।।

a granthir granthanāt smṛtaḥ
doṣāsra-māṃsa-medo-'sthi-sirā-vraṇa-bhavā nava ।
te tatra vātād āyāma-toda-bhedānvito asitaḥ ।।

sthānāt sthānāntara-gatir a-kasmād dhāni-vṛddhi-mān ।
mṛdur vastir ivānaddho vibhinno acchaṃ sravaty asṛk ।।

pittāt sa-dāhaḥ pītābho rakto vā pacyate drutam ।
bhinno asram uṣṇaṃ sravati śleṣmaṇā nī-rujo ghanaḥ ।।

śītaḥ sa-varṇaḥ kaṇḍū-mān pakvaḥ pūyaṃ sraved ghanam ।
doṣair duṣṭe asṛji granthir bhaven mūrchatsu jantuṣu ।।

sirā-māṃsaṃ ca saṃśritya sa-svāpaḥ pitta-lakṣaṇaḥ ।
māṃsalair dūṣitaṃ māṃsam āhārair granthim āvahet ।।

snigdhaṃ mahāntaṃ kaṭhinaṃ sirā-naddhaṃ kaphākṛtim ।
pravṛddhaṃ medurair medo nītaṃ māṃse atha-vā tvaci ।।

vāyunā kurute granthiṃ bhṛśaṃ snigdhaṃ mṛduṃ calam ।
śleṣma-tulyākṛtiṃ deha-kṣaya-vṛddhi-kṣayodayam ।।

sa vibhinno ghanaṃ medas tāmrāsita-sitaṃ sravet ।
asthi-bhaṅgābhighātābhyām unnatāvanataṃ tu yat ।।

a vibhinno ghanaṃ medaḥ ūyaṃ tāmrāsitaṃ sravet 
asthi-bhagnābhighātābhyām
so asthi-granthiḥ padātes tu sahasāmbho-'vagāhanāt ।
vyāyāmād vā pratāntasya sirā-jālaṃ sa-śoṇitam ।।

vāyuḥ saṃpīḍya saṃkocya vakrī-kṛtya viśoṣya ca ।
niḥ-sphuraṃ nī-rujaṃ granthiṃ kurute sa sirāhvayaḥ ।।

āyuḥ prapīḍya saṃkocya
a-rūḍhe rūḍha-mātre vā vraṇe sarva-rasāśinaḥ ।
sārdre vā bandha-rahite gātre aśmābhihate atha-vā ।।

vāto asram a-srutaṃ duṣṭaṃ saṃśoṣya grathitaṃ vraṇam ।
kuryāt sa-dāhaḥ kaṇḍū-mān vraṇa-granthir ayaṃ smṛtaḥ ।।

āyuḥ prakupitaḥ kṣipraṃ rāpya marmāśritaṃ vraṇam
sādhyā doṣāsra-medo-jā na tu sthūla-kharāś calāḥ ।
marma-kaṇṭhodara-sthāś ca mahat tu granthito arbudam ।।

a tu sthūlāḥ kharāś calāḥ ahāṃs tu granthito arbudam
tal-lakṣaṇaṃ ca medo-'ntaiḥ ṣo-ḍhā doṣādibhis tu tat ।
prāyo medaḥ-kaphāḍhya-tvāt sthira-tvāc ca na pacyate ।।

sirā-sthaṃ śoṇitaṃ doṣaḥ saṃkocyāntaḥ prapīḍya ca ।
pācayeta tad ānaddhaṃ sāsrāvaṃ māṃsa-piṇḍitam ।।

aṃkocyānu prapīḍya ca aṃkocyānu prapīḍya vā aṃkocyāntaḥ prapīḍya vā 
a-srāvaṃ māṃsa-piṇḍa-tām
māṃsāṅkuraiś citaṃ yāti vṛddhiṃ cāśu sravet tataḥ ।
ajasraṃ duṣṭa-rudhiraṃ bhūri tac choṇitārbudam ।।

ṛddhaṃ cāśu sravet tataḥ
teṣv asṛṅ-māṃsa-je varjye catvāry anyāni sādhayet ।
prasthitā vaṅkṣaṇorv-ādim adhaḥ-kāyaṃ kapholbaṇāḥ ।।

doṣā māṃsāsra-gāḥ pādau kālenāśritya kurvate ।
śanaiḥ śanair ghanaṃ śophaṃ ślīpadaṃ tat pracakṣate ।।

ślīpadaṃ tat pracakṣyate
paripoṭa-yutaṃ kṛṣṇam a-nimitta-rujaṃ kharam ।
rūkṣaṃ ca vātāt pittāt tu pītaṃ dāha-jvarānvitam ।।

ūkṣaṃ ca vātāt pittāc ca ūkṣaṃ ca ślīpadaṃ vātāt 
pittād dāha-jvarānvitam
kaphād guru snigdham a-ruk citaṃ māṃsāṅkurair bṛhat ।
tat tyajed vatsarātītaṃ su-mahat su-parisruti ।।

itaṃ māṃsāṅkurair mahat
pāṇi-nāsauṣṭha-karṇeṣu vadanty eke tu pāda-vat ।
ślīpadaṃ jāyate tac ca deśe anūpe bhṛśaṃ bhṛśam ।।

adanty anye tu pāda-vat
meda-sthāḥ kaṇṭha-manyākṣa-kakṣā-vaṅkṣaṇa-gā malāḥ ।
sa-varṇān kaṭhinān snigdhān vārtākāmalakākṛtīn ।।

eda-sthāḥ kaṇṭha-manyākṣi-
avagāḍhān bahūn gaṇḍāṃś cira-pākāṃś ca kurvate ।
pacyante alpa-rujas te anye sravanty anye ati-kaṇḍurāḥ ।।

acyante alpa-rujas tv anye ravanty anye ati-kaṇḍulāḥ
naśyanty anye bhavanty anye dīrgha-kālānubandhinaḥ ।
gaṇḍa-mālāpacī ceyaṃ dūrveva kṣaya-vṛddhi-bhāk ।।

tāṃ tyajet sa-jvara-cchardi-pārśva-ruk-kāsa-pīnasām ।
a-bhedāt pakva-śophasya vraṇe cā-pathya-sevinaḥ ।।

-pārśva-ruk-śvāsa-pīnasām raṇe vā-pathya-sevinaḥ
anupraviśya māṃsādīn dūraṃ pūyo abhidhāvati ।
gatiḥ sā dūra-gamanān nāḍī nāḍīva saṃsruteḥ ।।

nāḍy ekān-ṛjur anyeṣāṃ saivāneka-gatir gatiḥ ।
sā doṣaiḥ pṛthag eka-sthaiḥ śalya-hetuś ca pañcamī ।।

oṣaiḥ pṛthak samastaiś ca
vātāt sa-ruk sūkṣma-mukhī vi-varṇā phenilodvamā ।
sravaty abhyadhikaṃ rātrau pittāt tṛḍ-jvara-dāha-kṛt ।।

pītoṣṇa-pūti-pūya-srud divā cāti niṣiñcati ।
ghana-picchila-saṃsrāvā kaṇḍūlā kaṭhinā kaphāt ।।

ītoṣṇa-pūti-pūyaṃ tu ītoṣṇa-pūti-pūyāśru v
pītoṣṇa-pūti-pūyāsrur
niśi cābhyadhika-kledā sarvaiḥ sarvākṛtiṃ tyajet ।।

arvaiḥ sarvākṛtis tyajet antaḥ-sthitaṃ śalyam an-āhṛtaṃ tu karoti nāḍīṃ vahate ca sāsya ।।

aroti nāḍīṃ vahate ca sāsyāt phenānuviddhaṃ tanum alpam uṣṇaṃ sāsraṃ ca pūyaṃ sa-rujaṃ ca nityam ।।

henānuviddhaṃ tanum accham uṣṇaṃ

uttarasthāna
granthiṣv āmeṣu kartavyā yathā-svaṃ śopha-vat kriyā ।
bṛhatī-citraka-vyāghrī-kaṇā-siddhena sarpiṣā ।।

snehayec chuddhi-kāmaṃ ca tīkṣṇaiḥ śuddhasya lepanam ।
saṃsvedya bahu-śo granthiṃ vimṛdnīyāt punaḥ punaḥ ।।

eṣa vāte viśeṣeṇa kramaḥ pittāsra-je punaḥ ।
jalaukaso himaṃ sarvaṃ kapha-je vātiko vidhiḥ ।।

tathāpy a-pakvaṃ chittvainaṃ sthite rakte agninā dahet ।
sādhv a-śeṣaṃ sa-śeṣo hi punar āpyāyate dhruvam ।।

unar ānahyate drutam
māṃsa-vraṇodbhavau granthī yāpayed evam eva ca ।
kāryaṃ medo-bhave apy etat taptaiḥ phalādibhiś ca tam ।।

āṭayed evam eva ca
pramṛdyāt tila-digdhena cchannaṃ dvi-guṇa-vāsasā ।
śastreṇa pāṭayitvā vā dahen medasi sūddhṛte ।।

ramṛjyāt tila-digdhena ahen medasi tūddhṛte
sirā-granthau nave peyaṃ tailaṃ sāhacaraṃ tathā ।
upanāho anila-harair vasti-karma sirā-vyadhaḥ ।।

arbude granthi-vat kuryāt yathā-svaṃ su-tarāṃ hitam ।
ślīpade anila-je vidhyet snigdha-svinnopanāhite ।।
ajā-śakṛc-chigru-mūla-lākṣā-surasa-kāñjikaiḥ ।।
-lākṣā-rasa-sa-kāñjikaiḥ -lavaṇa-kṣāra-kāñjikaiḥ
upodakā-pattra-piṇḍyā chadair ācchāditaṃ ghanam ।
niveśya paṭṭaṃ badhnīyāc chāmyaty evaṃ navārbudam ।।

upodakārka-piṇyāka- -cchadair ācchāditaṃ ghanam
jīrṇe cārka-cchada-sudhā-sāmudra-guḍa-kāñjikaiḥ ।
pracchāne piṇḍikā baddhā granthy-arbuda-vilāyanī ।।

jīrṇārdrārka-cchada-sudhā- -sāmudraṃ tulyakāmbubhiḥ pracchanne piṭikāṃ baddhvā pracchānair piṇḍikāṃ baddhvā 
granthy-arbuda-vilāyanam
sirām upari gulphasya dvy-aṅgule pāyayec ca tam ।
māsam eraṇḍa-jaṃ tailaṃ go-mūtreṇa samanvitam ।।

jīrṇe jīrṇānnam aśnīyāc chuṇṭhī-śṛta-payo-'nvitam ।
traivṛtaṃ vā pibed evam a-śāntāv agninā dahet ।।

gulphasyādhaḥ sirā-mokṣaḥ paitte sarvaṃ ca pitta-jit ।
sirām aṅguṣṭhake viddhvā kapha-je śīlayed yavān ।।

sa-kṣaudrāṇi kaṣāyāṇi vardhamānās tathābhayāḥ ।
limpet sarṣapa-vārtākī-mūlābhyāṃ dhanvayātha-vā ।।

-mūlābhyāṃ dhānyayātha-vā
ūrdhvādhaḥ-śodhanaṃ peyam apacyāṃ sādhitaṃ ghṛtam ।
dantī-dravantī-trivṛtā-jālinī-devadālibhiḥ ।।

śīlayet kapha-medo-ghnaṃ dhūma-gaṇḍūṣa-nāvanam ।
sirayāpahared raktaṃ piben mūtreṇa tārkṣya-jam ।।

palam ardha-palaṃ vāpi karṣaṃ vāpy uṣṇa-vāriṇā ।
kāñcanāra-tvacaṃ pītvā gaṇḍa-mālāṃ vyapohati ।।

karṣaṃ voṣṇena vāriṇā
granthīn a-pakvān ālimpen nākulī-paṭu-nāgaraiḥ ।
svinnān lavaṇa-poṭalyā kaṭhinān anu mardayet ।।

śamī-mūlaka-śigrūṇāṃ bījaiḥ sa-yava-sarṣapaiḥ ।
lepaḥ piṣṭo ṇmla-takreṇa granthi-gaṇḍa-vilāyanaḥ ।।

śamī-mūlaka-śigrūttha- śamī-mūlaka-śigrūmā- -bījaḥ sa-yava-sarṣapaiḥ 
-bījaiḥ sa-yava-sarṣapaiḥ
kṣuṇṇāni nimba-pattrāṇi kḷptair bhallātakaiḥ saha ।
śarāva-saṃpuṭe dagdhvā sārdhaṃ siddhārthakaiḥ samaiḥ ।।

jīrṇāni nimba-pattrāṇi klinnair bhallātakaiḥ saha
kṣiprair bhallātakaiḥ saha
etac chāgāmbunā piṣṭaṃ gaṇḍa-mālā-pralepanam ।।

gaṇḍa-mālā-vilepanam
pākon-mukhān srutāsrasya pitta-śleṣma-harair jayet ।
a-pakvān evo voddhṛtya kṣārāgnibhyām upācaret ।।

kākādanī-lāṅgalikā-nahikottuṇḍikī-phalaiḥ ।
jīmūta-bīja-karkoṭī-viśālā-kṛtavedhanaiḥ ।।

-nalikottuṇḍikī-phalaiḥ -nalikottuṇḍakī-phalaiḥ 
-nahikottaiṇḍukī-phalaiḥ
pāṭhānvitaiḥ palārdhāṃśair viṣa-karṣa-yutaiḥ pacet ।
prasthaṃ karañja-tailasya nirguṇḍī-sva-rasāḍhake ।।

athyānvitaiḥ palārdhāṃśair
anena mālā gaṇḍānāṃ cira-jā pūya-vāhinī ।
sidhyaty a-sādhya-kalpāpi pānābhyañjana-nāvanaiḥ ।।

tailaṃ lāṅgalikī-kanda-kalka-pādaṃ catur-guṇe ।
nirguṇḍī-sva-rase pakvaṃ nasyādyair apacī-praṇut ।।

-kalka-pāde catur-guṇe
bhadraśrī-dāru-marica-dvi-haridrā-trivṛd-ghanaiḥ ।
manaḥśilāla-nalada-viśālā-karavīrakaiḥ ।।

c bhadra-śrīdāru-marica- anaḥśilāla-madana-
go-mūtra-piṣṭaiḥ palikair viṣasyārdha-palena ca ।
brāhmī-rasārka-ja-kṣīra-go-śakṛd-rasa-saṃyutam ।।

prasthaṃ sarṣapa-tailasya siddham āśu vyapohati ।
pānādyaiḥ śīlitaṃ kuṣṭha-duṣṭa-nāḍī-vraṇāpacīḥ ।।

ānādyaiḥ śīlitaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ uṣṭa-nāḍī-vraṇāpacīḥ
vacā-harītakī-lākṣā-kaṭu-rohiṇi-candanaiḥ ।
tailaṃ prasādhitaṃ pītaṃ sa-mūlām apacīṃ jayet ।।

śarapuṅkhodbhavaṃ mūlaṃ piṣṭaṃ taṇḍula-vāriṇā ।
nasyāl lepāc ca duṣṭārur-apacī-viṣa-jantu-jit ।।

mūlair uttamakāraṇyāḥ pīluparṇyāḥ sahācarāt ।
sa-lodhrābhaya-yaṣṭy-āhva-śatāhvā-dvīpi-dārubhiḥ ।।

ūlair uttamavāruṇyāḥ ūlair uttaravāruṇyāḥ 
mūlair uttaravāriṇyāḥ
tailaṃ kṣīra-samaṃ siddhaṃ nasye abhyaṅge ca pūjitam ।
go-'vy-ajāśva-khurā dagdhāḥ kaṭu-tailena lepanam ।।

o-gajāśva-khurā dagdhāḥ
aiṅgudena tu kṛṣṇāhir vāyaso vā svayaṃ mṛtaḥ ।
ity a-śāntau gadasyānya-pārśva-jaṅghā-samāśritam ।।

ty a-śāntau gade cānya- -pārśve jaṅghā-samāśritam
vaster ūrdhvam adhas-tād vā medo hṛtvāgninā dahet ।
sthitasyordhvaṃ padaṃ mitvā tan-mānena ca pārṣṇitaḥ ।।
tata ūrdhvaṃ hared granthīn ity āha bhaga-vān nimiḥ ।।pārṣṇiṃ prati dvā-daśa cāṅgulāni muktvendra-vastiṃ ca gadānya-pārśve ।।vidārya matsyāṇḍa-nibhāni madhyāj jālāni karṣed iti suśrutoktiḥ ।।
ā-gulpha-karṇāt su-mitasya jantos tasyāṣṭa-bhāgaṃ khuḍakād vibhajya ।
ghrāṇārjave adhaḥ sura-rāja-vaster bhittvākṣa-mātraṃ tv apare vadanti ।।

hoṇārjave adhaḥ sura-rāja-vaster hittvākṣa-mātrām apare 
vadanti
upanāhyānilān nāḍīṃ pāṭitāṃ sādhu lepayet ।
pratyakpuṣpī-phala-yutais tailaiḥ piṣṭaiḥ sa-saindhavaiḥ ।।

paittīṃ tu tila-mañjiṣṭhā-nāgadantī-niśā-dvayaiḥ ।
ślaiṣmikīṃ tila-saurāṣṭrī-nikumbhāriṣṭa-saindhavaiḥ ।।

śalya-jāṃ tila-madhv-ājyair lepayec chinna-śodhitām ।
a-śastra-kṛtyām eṣiṇyā bhittvānte samyag-eṣitām ।।

kṣāra-pītena sūtreṇa bahu-śo dārayed gatim ।
vraṇeṣu duṣṭa-sūkṣmāsya-gambhīrādiṣu sādhanam ।।

ahu-śo pūrayed gatim
yā vartyo yāni tailāni tan nāḍīṣv api śasyate ।
piṣṭaṃ cañcu-phalaṃ lepān nāḍī-vraṇa-haraṃ param ।।

ghoṇṭā-phala-tvak lavaṇaṃ sa-lākṣaṃ būkasya pattraṃ vanitā-payaś ca ।
snug-arka-dugdhānvita eṣa kalko vartī-kṛto hanty a-cireṇa nāḍīm ।।

ukrasya pattraṃ vanitā-payaś ca ṛṣasya pattraṃ vanitā-payaś 
ca
sāmudra-sauvarcala-sindhu-janma-su-pakva-ghoṇṭā-phala-veśma-dhūmāḥ ।
āmrāta-gāyatri-ja-pallavāś ca kaṭaṅkaṭeryāv atha cetakī ca ।।

aṭaṅkaṭeryāv atha ketakī ca aṭaṅkaṭeryāv atha dīnikā ca
kalke abhyaṅge cūrṇe vartyāṃ caiteṣu śīlyamāneṣu ।
a-gatir iva naśyati gatiś capalā capaleṣu bhūtir iva ।।

artyāṃ caiteṣu sevyamāneṣu

uttarasthāna
snigdhā sa-varṇā grathitā nī-rujā mudga-saṃnibhā ।
piṭikā kapha-vātābhyāṃ bālānām ajagallikā ।।

nigdhāḥ sa-varṇā grathitā iṭikāḥ kapha-vātābhyāṃ ī-rujā mudga-saṃmitā 
ī-rujā mudga-saṃnibhāḥ
yava-prakhyā yava-prakhyā tābhyāṃ māṃsāśritā ghanā ।
a-vaktrā cālajī vṛttā stoka-pūyā ghanonnatā ।।

ava-prakhyā yavākārā -vaktrāś cālajī-vṛttāḥ 
stoka-pūyā ghanonnatāḥ
granthayaḥ pañca vā ṣaḍ vā kacchapī kacchaponnatāḥ ।
karṇasyordhvaṃ samantād vā piṭikā kaṭhinogra-ruk ।।

acchapī kacchaponnatā
śālūkābhā panasikā śophas tv alpa-rujaḥ sthiraḥ ।
hanu-saṃdhi-samudbhūtas tābhyāṃ pāṣāṇa-gardabhaḥ ।।

śālmalī-kaṇṭakākārāḥ piṭikāḥ sa-rujo ghanāḥ ।
medo-garbhā mukhe yūnāṃ tābhyāṃ ca mukha-dūṣikāḥ ।।

ābhyāṃ ca mukha-dūṣakāḥ
te padma-kaṇṭakā jñeyā yaiḥ padmam iva kaṇṭakaiḥ ।
cīyate nī-rujaiḥ śvetaiḥ śarīraṃ kapha-vāta-jaiḥ ।।

pittena piṭikā vṛttā pakvodumbara-saṃnibhā ।
mahā-dāha-jvara-karī vivṛtā vivṛtānanā ।।

gātreṣv antaś ca vaktrasya dāha-jvara-rujānvitāḥ ।
masūra-mātrās tad-varṇās tat-saṃjñāḥ piṭikā ghanāḥ ।।

tataḥ kaṣṭa-tarāḥ sphoṭā visphoṭākhyā mahā-rujāḥ ।
yā padma-karṇikākārā piṭikā piṭikācitā ।।

sā viddhā vāta-pittābhyāṃ tābhyām eva ca gardabhī ।
maṇḍalā vipulotsannā sa-rāga-piṭikācitā ।।

kakṣeti kakṣāsanneṣu prāyo deśeṣu sānilāt ।
pittād bhavanti piṭikāḥ sūkṣmā lājopamā ghanāḥ ।।

ūkṣmā jālopamā ghanāḥ
tādṛśī mahatī tv ekā gandha-nāmeti kīrtitā ।
gharma-sveda-parīte aṅge piṭikāḥ sa-rujo ghanāḥ ।।

rājīkā-varṇa-saṃsthāna-pramāṇā rājikāhvayāḥ ।
doṣaiḥ pittolbaṇair mandair visarpati visarpa-vat ।।

śopho a-pākas tanus tāmro jvara-kṛj jāla-gardabhaḥ ।
malaiḥ pittolbaṇaiḥ sphoṭā jvariṇo māṃsa-dāraṇāḥ ।।

variṇo māṃsa-dāruṇāḥ variṇo māṃsa-dāriṇaḥ
kakṣā-bhāgeṣu jāyante ye agny-ābhāḥ sāgni-rohiṇī ।
pañcāhāt sapta-rātrād vā pakṣād vā hanti jīvitam ।।

tri-liṅgā piṭikā vṛttā jatrūrdhvam irivellikā ।
vidārī-kanda-kaṭhinā vidārī kakṣa-vaṅkṣaṇe ।।

medo-'nila-kaphair granthiḥ snāyu-māṃsa-sirāśrayaiḥ ।
bhinno vasājya-madhv-ābhaṃ sravet tatrolbaṇo anilaḥ ।।

māṃsaṃ viśoṣya grathitāṃ śarkarāṃ upapādayet ।
dur-gandhaṃ rudhiraṃ klinnaṃ nānā-varṇaṃ tato malāḥ ।।

ur-gandhi rudhiraṃ klinnaṃ
tāṃ srāvayanti nicitāṃ vidyāt tac charkarārbudam ।
pāṇi-pāda-tale saṃdhau jatrūrdhvaṃ vopacīyate ।।

āṃ srāvayanti nicitā atrūrdhvaṃ copacīyate
valmīka-vac chanair granthis tad-vad bahv-aṇubhir mukhaiḥ ।
rug-dāha-kaṇḍū-kledāḍhyair valmīko asau samasta-jaḥ ।।

ug-dāha-kaṇḍū-kledāḍhyo
śarkaronmathite pāde kṣate vā kaṇṭakādibhiḥ ।
granthiḥ kīla-vad utsanno jāyate kadaraṃ tu tat ।।

vega-saṃdhāraṇād vāyur apāno apāna-saṃśrayam ।
aṇū-karoti bāhyāntar-mārgam asya tataḥ śakṛt ।।

pāno apāna-saṃśrayaḥ
kṛcchrān nirgacchati vyādhir ayaṃ ruddha-gudo mataḥ ।
kuryāt pittānilaṃ pākaṃ nakha-māṃse sa-rug-jvaram ।।

cipyam a-kṣata-rogaṃ ca vidyād upa-nakhaṃ ca tam ।
kṛṣṇo abhighātād rūkṣaś ca kharaś ca ku-nakho nakhaḥ ।।

idyād upa-nakhaṃ ca tat
duṣṭa-kardama-saṃsparśāt kaṇḍū-kledānvitāntarāḥ ।
aṅgulyo alasam ity āhus tilābhāṃs tila-kālakān ।।

kṛṣṇān a-vedanāṃs tvak-sthān māṣāṃs tān eva connatān ।
maṣebhyas tūnnata-tarāṃś carma-kīlān sitāsitān ।।

tathā-vidho jatu-maṇiḥ saha-jo lohitas tu saḥ ।
kṛṣṇaṃ sitaṃ vā saha-jaṃ maṇḍalaṃ lāñchanaṃ samam ।।

a-rujo lohitas tu saḥ
śoka-krodhādi-kupitād vāta-pittān mukhe tanu ।
śyāmalaṃ maṇḍalaṃ vyaṅgaṃ vaktrād anya-tra nīlikā ।।

paruṣaṃ paruṣa-sparśaṃ vyaṅgaṃ śyāvaṃ ca mārutāt ।
pittāt tāmrāntam ā-nīlaṃ śvetāntaṃ kaṇḍu-mat kaphāt ।।

ittāt tāmraṃ tathā nīlaṃ śvetābhaṃ kaṇḍu-mat kaphāt
raktād raktāntam ā-tāmraṃ sauṣaṃ cimicimāyate ।
vāyunodīritaḥ śleṣmā tvacaṃ prāpya viśuṣyati ।।

ukhaṃ cimicimāyate
tatas tvag jāyate pāṇduḥ krameṇa ca vi-cetanā ।
alpa-kaṇḍūr a-vikledā sā prasuptiḥ prasuptitaḥ ।।

lpa-kaṇḍūr apa-kledā
a-samyag-vamanodīrṇa-pitta-śleṣmānna-nigrahaiḥ ।
maṇḍalāny ati-kaṇḍūni rāga-vanti bahūni ca ।।

utkoṭhaḥ so anubaddhas tu koṭha ity abhidhīyate ।
proktāḥ ṣaṭ-triṃśad ity ete kṣudra-rogā vibhāga-śaḥ ।।

tkoṭhaḥ so anubandhas tu yān a-vijñāya muhyeta cikitsāyāṃ cikitsakaḥ ।।

uttarasthāna
visrāvayej jalaukobhir a-pakvām ajagallikām ।
svedayitvā yava-prakhyāṃ vilayāya pralepayet ।।

dāru-kuṣṭha-manohvālair ity ā-pāṣāṇa-gardabhāt ।
vidhis tāṃś cācaret pakvān vraṇa-vat sājagallikān ।।

lodhra-kustumburu-vacāḥ pralepo mukha-dūṣike ।
vaṭa-pallava-yuktā vā nārikelottha-śuktayaḥ ।।

odhra-kustumburu-vacā- -pralepo mukha-dūṣike
a-śāntau vamanaṃ nasyaṃ lalāṭe ca sirā-vyadhaḥ ।
nimbāmbu-vānto nimbāmbu-sādhitaṃ padma-kaṇṭake ।।
pibet kṣaudrānvitaṃ sarpir nimbāragvadha-lepanam ।।
imbāragvadha-lepanaḥ vivṛtādīṃs tu jālāntāṃś cikitset serivellikān ।।

ikitsed irivellikām pitta-visarpa-vat tad-vat pratyākhyāyāgni-rohiṇīm ।।

vilaṅghanaṃ rakta-vimokṣaṇaṃ ca virūkṣaṇaṃ kāya-viśodhanaṃ ca ।
dhātrī-prayogāñ chiśira-pradehān kuryāt sadā jālaka-gardabhasya ।।

irūkṣaṇaṃ kāya-virecanaṃ ca hātrī-pradehāñ chiśira-prayogān
vidārikāṃ hṛte rakte śleṣma-granthi-vad ācaret ।
medo-'rbuda-kriyāṃ kuryāt su-tarāṃ śarkarārbude ।।

pravṛddhaṃ su-bahu-cchidraṃ sa-śophaṃ marmaṇi sthitam ।
valmīkaṃ hasta-pāde ca varjayed itarat punaḥ ।।

arjayed itaraṃ punaḥ
śuddhasyāsre hṛte limpet sa-paṭv-ārevatāmṛtaiḥ ।
śyāmā-kulatthikā-mūla-dantī-palala-saktubhiḥ ।।

a-paṭv-āragvadhāmṛtaiḥ
pakve tu duṣṭa-māṃsāni gatīḥ sarvāś ca śodhayet ।
śastreṇa samyag anu ca kṣāreṇa jvalanena vā ।।

śastreṇotkṛtya niḥ-śeṣaṃ snehena kadaraṃ dahet ।
niruddha-maṇi-vat kāryaṃ ruddha-pāyoś cikitsitam ।।

śastreṇoddhṛtya niḥ-śeṣaṃ
cipyaṃ śuddhyā jitoṣmāṇaṃ sādhayec chastra-karmaṇā ।
duṣṭaṃ ku-nakham apy evaṃ caraṇāv alase punaḥ ।।

dhānyāmla-siktau kāsīsa-paṭolī-rocanā-tilaiḥ ।
sa-nimba-pattrair ālimped dahet tu tila-kālakān ।।

maṣāṃś ca sūrya-kāntena kṣāreṇa yadi vāgninā ।
tad-vad utkṛtya śastreṇa carma-kīla-jatū-maṇī ।।

lāñchanādi-traye kuryād yathāsannaṃ sirā-vyadham ।
lepayet kṣīra-piṣṭaiś ca kṣīri-vṛkṣa-tvag-aṅkuraiḥ ।।

yacchādi-tritaye kuryād
vyaṅgeṣu cārjuna-tvag vā mañjiṣṭhā vā sa-mākṣikā ।
lepaḥ sa-nava-nītā vā śvetāśva-khura-jā maṣī ।।

yaṅgeṣu vārjuna-tvag vā
rakta-candana-mañjiṣṭhā-kuṣṭha-lodhra-priyaṅgavaḥ ।
vaṭāṅkurā masūrāś ca vyaṅga-ghnā mukha-kānti-dāḥ ।।

dve jīrake kṛṣṇa-tilāḥ sarṣapāḥ payasā saha ।
piṣṭāḥ kurvanti vaktrendum apāsta-vyaṅga-lāñchanam ।।

kṣīra-piṣṭā ghṛta-kṣaudra-yuktā vā bhṛṣṭa-nis-tuṣāḥ ।
masūrāḥ kṣīra-piṣṭā vā tīkṣṇāḥ śālmali-kaṇṭakāḥ ।।

sa-guḍaḥ kola-majjā vā śaśāsṛk-kṣaudra-kalkitaḥ ।
saptāhaṃ mātuluṅga-sthaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ vā madhunānvitam ।।

uṣṭhaṃ vā madhukānvitam
piṣṭā vā chāga-payasā sa-kṣaudrā mausalī jaṭā ।
gor asthi musalī-mūla-yuktaṃ vā sājya-mākṣikam ।।

jambv-āmra-pallavā mastu haridre dve navo guḍaḥ ।
lepaḥ sa-varṇa-kṛt piṣṭaṃ sva-rasena ca tindukam ।।

utpalam utpala-kuṣṭhaṃ priyaṅgu-kālīyakaṃ badara-majjā ।
idam udvartanam āsyaṃ karoti śatapattra-saṃkāśam ।।

tpala-pattraṃ tagaraṃ aroti śatapattrakākāram
ebhir evauṣadhaiḥ piṣṭair mukhābhyaṅgāya sādhayet ।
yathā-doṣartukān snehān madhuka-kvātha-saṃyutaiḥ ।।

yavān sarja-rasaṃ lodhram uśīraṃ madanaṃ madhu ।
ghṛtaṃ guḍaṃ ca go-mūtre paced ā-darvi-lepanāt ।।

śīraṃ candanaṃ madhu
tad abhyaṅgān nihanty āśu nīlikā-vyaṅga-dūṣikān ।
mukhaṃ karoti padmābhaṃ pādau padma-dalopamau ।।

īlikā-vyaṅga-dūṣakān
kuṅkumośīra-kālīya-lākṣā-yaṣṭy-āhva-candanam ।
nyagrodha-pādāṃs taruṇān padmakaṃ padma-kesaram ।।

sa-nīlotpala-mañjiṣṭhaṃ pālikaṃ salilāḍhake ।
paktvā pādāvaśeṣeṇa tena piṣṭaiś ca kārṣikaiḥ ।।

lākṣā-pattaṅga-mañjiṣṭhā-yaṣṭīmadhuka-kuṅkumaiḥ ।
ajā-kṣīraṃ dvi-guṇitaṃ tailasya kuḍavaṃ pacet ।।

jā-kṣīra-dvi-guṇitaṃ
nīlikā-palita-vyaṅga-valī-tilaka-dūṣikān ।
hanti tan nasyam abhyastaṃ mukhopacaya-varṇa-kṛt ।।
mañjiṣṭhā śabarodbhavas tubarikā lākṣā haridrā-dvayaṃ ।।nepālī haritāla-kuṅkuma-gadā go-rocanā gairikam ।।
epālī haritāla-kuṅkuma-gadaṃ go-rocanā gairikam pattraṃ pāṇḍu vaṭasya candana-yugaṃ kālīyakaṃ pāradaṃ ।।
pattaṅgaṃ kanaka-tvacaṃ kamala-jaṃ bījaṃ tathā kesaram ।।
sikthaṃ tutthaṃ padmakādyo vasājyaṃ majjā kṣīraṃ kṣīri-vṛkṣāmbu cāgnau ।
siddhaṃ siddhaṃ vyaṅga-nīly-ādi-nāśe vaktre chāyām aindavīṃ cāśu dhatte ।।

mārkava-sva-rasa-kṣīra-toyānīṣṭāni nāvane ।
prasuptau vāta-kuṣṭhoktaṃ kuryād dāhaṃ ca vahninā ।।

-toya-piṣṭāni nāvane utkoṭhe kapha-pittoktaṃ koṭhe sarvaṃ ca kauṣṭhikam ।।

uttarasthāna
strī-vyavāya-nivṛttasya sahasā bhajato atha-vā ।
doṣādhyuṣita-saṃkīrṇa-malināṇu-rajaḥ-pathām ।।

trīṃ vyavāya-nivṛttasya
anya-yonim an-icchantīm a-gamyāṃ nava-sūtikām ।
dūṣitaṃ spṛśatas toyaṃ ratānteṣv api naiva vā ।।

vivardhayiṣayā tīkṣṇān pralepādīn prayacchataḥ ।
muṣṭi-danta-nakhotpīḍā-viṣa-vac-chūka-pātanaiḥ ।।

-viṣa-val-lūka-pātanaiḥ
vega-nigraha-dīrghāti-khara-sparśa-vighaṭṭanaiḥ ।
doṣā duṣṭā gatā guhyaṃ trayo-viṃśatim āmayān ।।

-khara-sparśādi-ghaṭṭanaiḥ -khara-śaṣpādi-ghaṭṭanaiḥ
janayanty upadaṃśādīn upadaṃśo atra pañca-dhā ।
pṛthag doṣaiḥ sa-rudhiraiḥ samastaiś cātra mārutāt ।।

anayanty avadaṃśādīn vadaṃśo atra pañca-dhā
meḍhre śopho rujaś citrāḥ stambhas tvak-paripoṭanam ।
pakvodumbara-saṃkāśaḥ pittena śvayathur jvaraḥ ।।

eḍhra-śopho rujaś citrāḥ
śleṣmaṇā kaṭhinaḥ snigdhaḥ kaṇḍū-māñ chītalo guruḥ ।
śoṇitenāsita-sphoṭa-saṃbhavo asra-srutir jvaraḥ ।।

sarva-je sarva-liṅga-tvaṃ śvayathur muṣkayor api ।
tīvrā rug āśu-pacanaṃ daraṇaṃ kṛmi-saṃbhavaḥ ।।

āraṇaṃ kṛmi-saṃbhavaḥ
yāpyo raktodbhavas teṣāṃ mṛtyave saṃnipāta-jaḥ ।
jāyante kupitair doṣair guhyāsṛk-piśitāśrayaiḥ ।।

antar bahir vā meḍhrasya kaṇḍūlā māṃsa-kīlakāḥ ।
picchilāsra-sravā yonau tad-vac ca cchattra-saṃnibhāḥ ।।

te arśāṃsy upekṣayā ghnanti meḍhra-puṃs-tvaṃ bhagārtavaṃ ।
guhyasya bahir antar vā piṭikāḥ kapha-rakta-jāḥ ।।

eḍhra-puṃs-tva-bhagārtavaṃ eḍhraṃ puṃso bhagārtavaṃ
sarṣapā-māna-saṃsthānā ghanāḥ sarṣapikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
piṭikā bahavo dīrghā dīryante madhyataś ca yāḥ ।।

so avamanthaḥ kaphāsṛgbhyāṃ vedanā-roma-harṣa-vān ।
kumbhīkā rakta-pittotthā jāmbavāsthi-nibhāśu-jā ।।

āmbavāsthi-nibhā-śubhā
alajīṃ meha-vad vidyād uttamāṃ pitta-rakta-jām ।
piṭikāṃ māṣa-mudgābhāṃ piṭikā piṭikācitā ।।

ttamāṃ rakta-pitta-jām
karṇikā puṣkarasyeva jñeyā puṣkariketi sā ।
pāṇibhyāṃ bhṛśa-saṃvyūḍhe saṃvyūḍha-piṭikā bhavet ।।

mṛditaṃ mṛditaṃ vastra-saṃrabdhaṃ vāta-kopataḥ ।
viṣamā kaṭhinā bhugnā vāyunāṣṭhīlikā smṛtā ।।

ṛditaṃ mṛditaṃ yat tu ṛditaṃ mṛditaṃ vastu 
saṃrabdhaṃ vāta-kopataḥ
vimardanādi-duṣṭena vāyunā carma meḍhra-jam ।
nivartate sa-rug-dāhaṃ kva-cit pākaṃ ca gacchati ।।

va-cit pākaṃ na gacchati
piṇḍitaṃ granthitaṃ carma tat pralambam adho maṇeḥ ।
nivṛtta-saṃjñaṃ sa-kaphaṃ kaṇḍū-kāṭhinya-vat tu tat ।।

iṇḍitaṃ granthitaṃ tac ca ipralambam adho maṇeḥ 
pravilambam adho maṇeḥ
dur-ūḍhaṃ sphuṭitaṃ carma nirdiṣṭam avapāṭikā ।
vātena dūṣitaṃ carma maṇau saktaṃ ruṇaddhi cet ।।

uḥ-sahaṃ sphuṭitaṃ carma aṇau saktaṃ ruṇaddhi tat
sroto mūtraṃ tato abhyeti manda-dhāram a-vedanam ।
maṇer vikāśa-rodhaś ca sa niruddha-maṇir gadaḥ ।।

liṅgaṃ śūkair ivāpūrṇaṃ grathitākhyaṃ kaphodbhavam ।
śūka-dūṣita-raktotthā sparśa-hānis tad-āhvayā ।।

chidrair aṇu-mukhair yat tu mehanaṃ sarvataś citam ।
vāta-śoṇita-kopena taṃ vidyāc chata-ponakam ।।

pittāsṛgbhyāṃ tvacaḥ pākas tvak-pāko jvara-dāha-vān ।
māṃs-pākaḥ sarva-jaḥ sarva-vedano māṃsa-śātanaḥ ।।

sa-rāgair asitaiḥ sphoṭaiḥ piṭikābhiś ca pīḍitam ।
mehanaṃ vedanā cogrā taṃ vidyād asṛg-arbudam ।।

māṃsārbudaṃ prāg uditaṃ vidradhiś ca tri-doṣa-jaḥ ।
kṛṣṇāni bhūtvā māṃsāni viśīryante samantataḥ ।।

pakvāni saṃnipātena tān vidyāt tila-kālakān ।
māṃsottham arbudaṃ pākaṃ vidradhiṃ tila-kālakān ।।

caturo varjayed eṣāṃ śeṣāñ chīghram upācaret ।
viṃśatir vyāpado yoner jāyante duṣṭa-bhojanāt ।।

viṣama-sthāṅga-śayana-bhṛśa-maithuna-sevanaiḥ ।
duṣṭārtavād apadravair bīja-doṣeṇa daivataḥ ।।

uṣṭārtavād upadravair
yonau kruddho anilaḥ kuryād ruk-todāyāma-supta-tāḥ ।
pipīlikā-sṛptim iva stambhaṃ karkaśa-tāṃ svanam ।।

ipīlikā-gatim iva
phenilāruṇa-kṛṣṇālpa-tanu-rūkṣārtava-srutim ।
sraṃsaṃ vaṅkṣaṇa-pārśvādau vyathāṃ gulmaṃ krameṇa ca ।।

ūru-vaṅkṣaṇa-pārśvādau hṛśaṃ vaṅkṣaṇa-pārśvādau
tāṃs tāṃś ca svān gadān vyāpad vātikī nāma sā smṛtā ।
saivāti-caraṇā śopha-saṃyuktāti-vyavāyataḥ ।।

āṃs tāṃś ca sva-gadān vyāpad āṃs tān svāṃs svān gadān 
vyāpad
maithunād ati-bālāyāḥ pṛṣṭha-jaṅghoru-vaṅkṣaṇam ।
rujan saṃdūṣayed yoniṃ vāyuḥ prāk-caraṇeti sā ।।

vegodāvartanād yoniṃ prapīḍayati mārutaḥ ।
sā phenilaṃ rajaḥ kṛcchrād udāvṛttaṃ vimuñcati ।।

egenāvartanād yoniṃ dāvartaṃ vimuñcati 
udāvartya vimuñcati
iyaṃ vyāpad udāvṛttā jāta-ghnī tu yadānilaḥ ।
jātaṃ jātaṃ sutaṃ hanti raukṣyād duṣṭārtavodbhavam ।।

yaṃ vyāpad udāvartā
aty-āśitāyā viṣamaṃ sthitāyāḥ su-rate marut ।
annenotpīḍito yoneḥ sthitaḥ srotasi vakrayet ।।

sāsthi-māṃsaṃ mukhaṃ tīvra-rujam antar-mukhīti sā ।
vātalāhāra-sevinyāṃ jananyāṃ kupito anilaḥ ।।

-rujaṃ vakra-mukhīti sā
striyo yonim aṇu-dvārāṃ kuryāt sūcī-mukhīti sā ।
vega-rodhād ṛtau vāyur duṣṭo viṇ-mūtra-saṃgraham ।।

karoti yoneḥ śoṣaṃ ca śuṣkākhyā sāti-vedanā ।
ṣaḍ-ahāt sapta-rātrād vā śukraṃ garbhāśayān marut ।।

vamet sa-ruṅ nī-rujo vā yasyāḥ sā vāminī matā ।
yonau vātopataptāyāṃ strī-garbhe bīja-doṣataḥ ।।

amet sa-ruṅ nī-rujo vā hy asyāṃ sā vāminī matā 
asyāṃ sā vāminī matā
nṛ-dveṣiṇy a-stanī ca syāt ṣaṇḍha-saṃjñān-upakramā ।
duṣṭo viṣṭabhya yony-āsyaṃ garbha-koṣṭhaṃ ca mārutaḥ ।।

kurute vivṛtāṃ srastāṃ vātikīm iva duḥkhitām ।
utsanna-māṃsāṃ tām āhur mahā-yoniṃ mahā-rujām ।।

yathā-svair dūṣaṇair duṣṭaṃ pittaṃ yonim upāśritam ।
karoti dāha-pākoṣā-pūti-gandhi-jvarānvitām ।।

-pūti-gandha-jvarānvitām -pūti-gandhāṃ jvarānvitām
bhṛśoṣṇa-bhūri-kuṇapa-nīla-pītāsitārtavām ।
sā vyāpat paittikī rakta-yony-ākhyāsṛg-ati-sruteḥ ।।

kapho abhiṣyandibhiḥ kruddhaḥ kuryād yonim a-vedanām ।
śītalāṃ kaṇḍulāṃ pāṇḍu-picchilāṃ tad-vidha-srutim ।।

sā vyāpac chlaiṣmikī vāta-pittābhyāṃ kṣīyate rajaḥ ।
sa-dāha-kārśya-vaivarṇyaṃ yasyāḥ sā lohita-kṣayā ।।

asyāṃ sā lohita-kṣayā
pittalāyā nṛ-saṃvāse kṣavathūdgāra-dhāraṇāt ।
pitta-yuktena marutā yonir bhavati dūṣitā ।।

śūnā sparśā-sahā sārtir nīla-pītāsra-vāhinī ।
vasti-kukṣi-guru-tvātīsārā-rocaka-kāriṇī ।।

śroṇi-vaṅkṣaṇa-ruk-toda-jvara-kṛt sā pariplutā ।
vāta-śleṣmāmaya-vyāptā śveta-picchila-vāhinī ।।

upaplutā smṛtā yonir viplutākhyā tv a-dhāvanāt ।
saṃjāta-jantuḥ kaṇḍūlā kaṇḍvā cāti-rati-priyā ।।

a-kāla-vāhanād vāyuḥ śleṣma-rakta-vimūrchitaḥ ।
karṇikāṃ janayed yonau rajo-mārga-nirodhinīm ।।

sā karṇinī tribhir doṣair yoni-garbhāśayāśritaiḥ ।
yathā-svopadrava-karair vyāpat sā sāṃnipātikī ।।

iti yoni-gadā nārī yaiḥ śukraṃ na pratīcchati ।
tato garbhaṃ na gṛhṇāti rogāṃś cāpnoti dāruṇān ।।
asṛg-darārśo-gulmādīn ābādhāṃś cānilādibhiḥ ।।
ū̆ābādhāś cānilādibhiḥ

uttarasthāna
meḍhra-madhye sirāṃ vidhyed upadaṃśe navotthite ।
śītāṃ kuryāt kriyāṃ śuddhiṃ virekeṇa viśeṣataḥ ।।

vadaṃśe navotthite
tila-kalka-ghṛta-kṣaudrair lepaḥ pakve tu pāṭite ।
jambv-āmra-sumano-nīpa-śveta-kāmbojikāṅkurān ।।

śallakī-badarī-bilva-palāśa-tiniśodbhavāḥ ।
tvacaḥ kṣīri-drumāṇāṃ ca tri-phalāṃ ca pacej jale ।।

sa kvāthaḥ kṣālanaṃ tena pakvaṃ tailaṃ ca ropaṇam ।
tuttha-gairika-lodhrailā-manohvāla-rasāñjanaiḥ ।।

a kvāthaḥ kṣālane tena
hareṇu-puṣpa-kāsīsa-saurāṣṭrī-lavaṇottamaiḥ ।
lepaḥ kṣaudra-drutaiḥ sūkṣmair upadaṃśa-vraṇāpahaḥ ।।

vadaṃśa-vraṇāpahaḥ
kapāle tri-phalā dagdhā sa-ghṛtā ropaṇaṃ param ।
sāmānyaṃ sādhanam idaṃ prati-doṣaṃ tu śopha-vat ।।

na ca yāti yathā pākaṃ prayateta tathā bhṛśam ।
pakvaiḥ snāyu-sirā-māṃsaiḥ prāyo naśyati hi dhvajaḥ ।।

arśasāṃ chinna-dagdhānāṃ kriyā kāryopadaṃśa-vat ।
sarṣapā likhitāḥ sūkṣmaiḥ kaṣāyair avacūrṇayet ।।

riyā kāryāvadaṃśa-vat arṣapāṃ likhitāṃ sūkṣmaiḥ
tair evābhyañjanaṃ tailaṃ sādhayed vraṇa-ropaṇam ।
kriyeyam avamanthe api raktaṃ srāvyaṃ tathobhayoḥ ।।

kumbhīkāyāṃ hared raktaṃ pakvāyāṃ śodhite vraṇe ।
tinduka-tri-phalā-lodhrair lepas tailaṃ ca ropaṇam ।।

alajyāṃ sruta-raktāyām ayam eva kriyā-kramaḥ ।
uttamākhyāṃ tu piṭikāṃ saṃchidya baḍiśoddhṛtām ।।

kalkaiś cūrṇaiḥ kaṣāyāṇāṃ kṣaudra-yuktair upācaret ।
kramaḥ pitta-visarpoktaḥ puṣkara-vyūḍhayor hitaḥ ।।

tvak-pāke sparśa-hānyāṃ ca secayed mṛditaṃ punaḥ ।
balā-tailena koṣṇena madhuraiś copanāhayet ।।

vak-pāke sparśa-hānyau vā
aṣṭhīlikāṃ hṛte rakte śleṣma-granthi-vad ācaret ।
nivṛttaṃ sarpiṣābhyajya svedayitvopanāhayet ।।

tri-rātraṃ pañca-rātraṃ vā su-snigdhaiḥ śālvaṇādibhiḥ ।
svedayitvā tato bhūyaḥ snigdhaṃ carma samānayet ।।

nigdhaṃ carma samāharet
maṇiṃ prapīḍya śanakaiḥ praviṣṭe copanāhanam ।
maṇau punaḥ punaḥ snigdhaṃ bhojanaṃ cātra śasyate ।।

ayam eva prayojyaḥ syād avapāṭyām api kramaḥ ।
nāḍīm ubhayato-dvārāṃ niruddhe jatunā sṛtām ।।

iruddhe jatunā śṛtām iruddhe jatunā kṛtām
snehāktāṃ srotasi nyasya siñcet snehaiś calāpahaiḥ ।
try-ahāt try-ahāt sthūla-tarāṃ nyasya nāḍīṃ vivardhayet ।।

sroto-dvāram a-siddhau tu vidvān śastreṇa pāṭayet ।
sevanīṃ varjayan yuñjyāt sadyaḥ-kṣata-vidhiṃ tataḥ ।।

roto-dvāram a-siddhau vā
granthitaṃ sveditaṃ nāḍyā snigdhoṣṇair upanāhayet ।
limpet kaṣāyaiḥ sa-kṣaudrair likhitvā śata-ponakam ।।

rakta-vidradhi-vat kāryā cikitsā śoṇitārbude ।
vraṇopacāraṃ sarveṣu yathāvasthaṃ prayojayet ।।

yoni-vyāpatsu bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śasyate karma vāta-jit ।
snehana-sveda-vasty-ādi vāta-jāsu viśeṣataḥ ।।

na hi vātād ṛte yonir vanitānāṃ praduṣyati ।
ato jitvā tam anyasya kuryād doṣasya bheṣajam ।।

to a-jitvā tam anyac ca to a-jitvā tam anyasya a 
kuryād doṣa-bheṣajam
pāyayeta balā-tailaṃ miśrakaṃ su-kumārakam ।
snigdha-svinnāṃ tathā yoniṃ duḥ-sthitāṃ sthāpayet samām ।।

āyayec ca balā-tailaṃ āyayet tāṃ balā-tailaṃ 
pāyayed vā balā-tailaṃ
pāṇinā namayej jihmāṃ saṃvṛtāṃ vyadhayet punaḥ ।
praveśayen niḥsṛtāṃ ca vivṛtāṃ parivartayet ।।

āṇinā nāmayej jihmāṃ āṇinonnamayej jihmāṃ 
saṃvṛtāṃ vyāsayet punaḥ
sthānāpavṛttā yonir hi śalya-bhūtā striyo matā ।
karmabhir vamanādyaiś ca mṛdubhir yojayet striyam ।।

thānāpavartā yonir hi
sarvataḥ su-viśuddhāyāḥ śeṣaṃ karma vidhīyate ।
vasty-abhyaṅga-parīṣeka-pralepa-picu-dhāraṇam ।।

arvatas tu viśuddhāyāḥ
kāśmarya-tri-phalā-drākṣā-kāsamarda-niśā-dvayaiḥ ।
guḍūcī-sairyakābhīru-śukanāsā-punarnavaiḥ ।।

uḍūcī-gairikābhīru-
parūṣakaiś ca vipacet prastham akṣa-samair ghṛtāt ।
yoni-vāta-vikāra-ghnaṃ tat pītaṃ garbha-daṃ param ।।

arūṣakaiś ca vipaced rastham akṣa-samair ghṛtam 
akṣaiḥ prastha-samaṃ ghṛtam
vacopakuñcikājājī-kṛṣṇā-vṛṣaka-saindhavam ।
ajamodā-yava-kṣāra-śarkarā-citrakānvitam ।।

piṣṭvā prasannayāloḍya khādet tad ghṛta-bharjitam ।
yoni-pārśvārti-hṛd-roga-gulmārśo-vinivṛttaye ।।

-gulmārśo-'rti-nivṛttaye
vṛṣakaṃ mātuluṅgasya mūlāni madayantikām ।
piben madyaiḥ sa-lavaṇais tathā kṛṣṇopakuñcike ।।

ṛṣasya mātuluṅgasya athā kṛṣṇopakuñcikā
rāsnā-śvadaṃṣṭrā-vṛṣakaiḥ śṛtaṃ śūla-haraṃ payaḥ ।
guḍūcī-tri-phalā-dantī-kvāthaiś ca pariṣecanam ।।

nata-vārtākinī-kuṣṭha-saindhavāmaradārubhiḥ ।
tailāt prasādhitād dhāryaḥ picur yonau rujāpahaḥ ।।

pittalānāṃ tu yonīnāṃ sekābhyaṅga-picu-kriyāḥ ।
śītāḥ pitta-jitaḥ kāryāḥ snehanārthaṃ ghṛtāni ca ।।

ittalānāṃ ca yonīnāṃ
śatāvarī-mūla-tulā-catuṣkāt kṣuṇṇa-pīḍitāt ।
rasena kṣīra-tulyena pācayeta ghṛtāḍhakam ।।

jīvanīyaiḥ śatāvaryā mṛdvīkābhiḥ parūṣakaiḥ ।
piṣṭaiḥ priyālaiś cākṣāṃśair dvi-balā-madhukānvitaiḥ ।।

adhukarddhi-balānvitaiḥ
siddha-śīte tu madhunaḥ pippalyāś ca palāṣṭakam ।
śarkarāyā daśa-palaṃ kṣipel lihyāt picuṃ tataḥ ।।

yony-asṛk-śukra-doṣa-ghnaṃ vṛṣyaṃ puṃ-savanaṃ param ।
kṣataṃ kṣayam asṛk-pittaṃ kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ halīmakam ।।

ṣata-kṣayam asṛk-pittaṃ
kāmalāṃ vāta-rudhiraṃ visarpaṃ hṛc-chiro-graham ।
apasmārārditāyāma-madonmādāṃś ca nāśayet ।।

pasmārārditāyāmān adonmādāṃś ca nāśayet
evam eva payaḥ-sarpir jīvanīyopasādhitam ।
garbha-daṃ pitta-jānāṃ ca rogāṇāṃ paramaṃ hitam ।।

balā-droṇa-dvaya-kvāthe ghṛta-tailāḍhakaṃ pacet ।
kṣīre catur-guṇe kṛṣṇā-kākanāsā-sitānvitaiḥ ।।

jīvantī-kṣīra-kākolī-sthirā-vīrarddhi-jīvakaiḥ ।
payasyā-śrāvaṇī-mudga-pīlu-māṣākhya-parṇibhiḥ ।।

-sthirā-vīrarddhi-jīrakaiḥ -sthirā-vīrā-dvi-jīvakaiḥ 
-pīlu-māṣākhukarṇibhiḥ
vāta-pittāmayān hatvā pānād garbhaṃ dadhāti tat ।
rakta-yonyām asṛg-varṇair anubandham avekṣya ca ।।

ānād garbhaṃ dadāti tat
yathā-doṣodayaṃ yuñjyād rakta-sthāpanam auṣadham ।
pāṭhāṃ jambv-āmrayor asthi śilodbhedaṃ rasāñjanam ।।

mañjiṣṭhāguru-kaṭphala-musta-priyaṅgu-miśi-kuṣṭhaiḥ ।
kaṭvaṅga-kuṭaja-śābara-kakubha-tvaṅ-madhuka-padmaka-madhūkaiḥ ।।

añjiṣṭhā-madhu-kaṭphala-
kuṅkuma-bilvātiviṣā-mākṣīka-rasāñjanaiḥ sa-kiñjalkaiḥ ।
piṣṭair ghṛtaṃ vipakvaṃ dvi-guṇāja-kṣīra-saṃyuktam ।।

strīṇām apatya-jananaṃ yoni-rujā-doṣa-jit sadā yuñjyāt ।
uttara-vastiṣu sarpir yojyaṃ kalyāṇakaṃ nāma ।।

ambaṣṭhāṃ śālmalī-picchāṃ samaṅgāṃ vatsaka-tvacam ।
bāhlīka-bilvātiviṣā-lodhra-toyada-gairikam ।।

amaṅgāṃ vatsaka-tvacām
śuṇṭhī-madhūka-mācīka-rakta-candana-kaṭphalam ।
kaṭvaṅga-vatsakānantā-dhātakī-madhukārjunam ।।

śuṇṭhī-madhuka-mācīka- śuṇṭhī-madhuka-mādhvīka- śuṇṭhī-madhuka-mārdvīka- śuṇṭhī-madhuka-mārdvīkā- śuṇṭhī-madhūka-mṛdvīkā- 
-dhātakī-madhukāñjanam
puṣye gṛhītvā saṃcūrṇya sa-kṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbhasā ।
pibed arśaḥsv atīsāre raktaṃ yaś copaveśyate ।।

a-kṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbunā
doṣā jantu-kṛtā ye ca bālānāṃ tāṃś ca nāśayet ।
yoni-doṣaṃ rajo-doṣaṃ śyāva-śvetāruṇāsitam ।।

oṣā danta-kṛtā ye ca
cūrṇaṃ puṣyānugaṃ nāma hitam ātreya-pūjitam ।
yonyāṃ balāsa-duṣṭāyāṃ sarvaṃ rūkṣoṣṇam auṣadham ।।

dhātaky-āmalakī-pattra-sroto-ja-madhukotpalaiḥ ।
jambv-āmra-sāra-kāsīsa-lodhra-kaṭphala-tindukaiḥ ।।

saurāṣṭrikā-dāḍima-tvag-udumbara-śalāṭubhiḥ ।
akṣa-mātrair ajā-mūtre kṣīre ca dvi-guṇe pacet ।।

taila-prasthaṃ tad abhyaṅga-picu-vastiṣu yojayet ।
tena śūnonnatā stabdhā picchilā srāviṇī tathā ।।

śūnottānonnatā stabdhā
viplutopaplutā yoniḥ sidhyet sa-sphoṭa-śūlinī ।
yavānnam abhayāriṣṭaṃ sīdhu tailaṃ ca śīlayet ।।

idhyeta sphoṭa-śūlinī
pippaly-ayo-rajaḥ-pathyā-prayogāṃś ca sa-mākṣikān ।
kāsīsaṃ tri-phalā kāṅkṣī sāmra-jambv-asthi dhātakī ।।

āsīsaṃ tri-phalā kācchī
paicchilye kṣaudra-saṃyuktaś cūrṇo vaiśadya-kārakaḥ ।
palāśa-dhātakī-jambū-samaṅgā-moca-sarja-jaḥ ।।

dur-gandhe picchile klede stambhanaś cūrṇa iṣyate ।
āragvadhādi-vargasya kaṣāyaḥ pariṣecanam ।।

aṣāyaḥ pariṣecane
stabdhānāṃ karkaśānāṃ ca kāryaṃ mārdava-kārakam ।
dhāraṇaṃ vesavārasya kṛśarā-pāyasasya ca ।।

dur-gandhānāṃ kaṣāyaḥ syāt tailaṃ vā kalka eva vā ।
cūrṇo vā sarva-gandhānāṃ pūti-gandhāpakarṣaṇaḥ ।।

ūti-gandhy-apakarṣaṇaḥ
śleṣmalānāṃ kaṭu-prāyāḥ sa-mūtrā vastayo hitāḥ ।
pitte sa-madhuka-kṣīrā vāte tailāmla-saṃyutāḥ ।।

saṃnipāta-samutthāyāḥ karma sādhāraṇaṃ hitam ।
evaṃ yoniṣu śuddhāsu garbhaṃ vindanti yoṣitaḥ ।।

aṃnipāta-samutthāyāṃ arbho bhavati yoṣitām
candano natayośīra-tiktā-padmebha-kesaraiḥ ।
kuṭaja-tvak-phalaṃ mustaṃ jambv-āmrāsthi rasāñjanam ।।

-tiktā-padmebha-kesaram
padmakotpala-bilvābda-kaṭphalaiḥ sādhitā niśā ।
dhātaky-ativiṣā-māṃsī-pāṭhā-moca-rasodakam ।।

madhūkaṃ madhukānantā-śārivā-dāḍima-[tva]cam ।
mṛl-lodhrārjuna-śaileya-samaṅgā nāgarāḥ samāḥ ।।

cūrṇaṃ śreṣṭhāmbunā pītaṃ hanti lohita-mehinam ।
mūrchā-tṛṣṇā-jvarārtāya raktātīsāra-mehinām ।।
strīṇām asṛg-daraṃ yāti garbha-saṃsthāpanaṃ param ।।
a-duṣṭe prākṛte bīje jīvopakramaṇe sati ।
pañca-karma-viśuddhasya puruṣasyāpi cendriyam ।।

parīkṣya varṇair doṣāṇāṃ duṣṭaṃ tad-ghnair upācaret ।
mañjiṣṭhā-kuṣṭha-tagara-tri-phalā-śarkarā-vacāḥ ।।

rasaṃ śirīṣa-pattrāṇāṃ kalkaṃ ca ṣaḍ-ahaḥ pibet ।
kṣīropanāśinā yoṣid ṛtu-snātā sutārthinī ।।

dve niśe madhukaṃ medāṃ dīpyakaṃ kaṭu-rohiṇīm ।
payasyā-hiṅgu-kākolī-vājigandhā-śatāvarīḥ ।।

ve niśe madhukaṃ medā īpyakaḥ kaṭu-rohiṇī ayasyā hiṅgu kākolī 
ājigandhā śatāvarī
piṣṭvākṣāṃśā ghṛta-prasthaṃ pacet kṣīra-catur-guṇam ।
yoni-śukra-pradoṣeṣu tat sarveṣu praśasyate ।।

iṣṭvākṣāṃśair ghṛta-prasthaṃ acet kṣīraṃ catur-guṇam acet kṣīre catur-guṇe 
at sarveṣu ca śasyate
āyuṣyaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ medhyaṃ dhanyaṃ puṃ-savanaṃ param ।
phala-sarpir iti khyātaṃ puṣpe pītaṃ phalāya yat ।।

mriyamāṇa-prajānāṃ ca garbhiṇīnāṃ ca pūjitam ।
etat paraṃ ca bālānāṃ graha-ghnaṃ deha-vardhanam ।।

uttarasthāna
mathyamāne jala-nidhāv amṛtārthaṃ surāsuraiḥ ।
jātaḥ prāg amṛtotpatteḥ puruṣo ghora-darśanaḥ ।।

dīpta-tejāś catur-daṃṣṭro hari-keśo analekṣaṇaḥ ।
jagad viṣaṇṇaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā tenāsau viṣa-saṃjñitaḥ ।।

arit-keśo analekṣaṇaḥ enāsau viṣa-saṃjñakaḥ
huṅ-kṛto brahmaṇā mūrtī tataḥ sthāvara-jaṅgame ।
so adhyatiṣṭhan nijaṃ rūpam ujjhitvā vañcanātmakam ।।

uṅ-kṛto brahmaṇā mūrtas uṅ-kṛto brahmaṇā mūrtīs ataḥ sthāvara-jaṅgamam ataḥ sthāvara-jaṅgamam ataḥ sthāvara-jaṅgamāt ataḥ sthāvara-jaṅgamāḥ 
jjhitvā vañcanātmakaḥ
sthiram ity ulbaṇaṃ vīrye yat kandeṣu pratiṣṭhitam ।
kālakūṭendravatsākhya-śṛṅgī-hālāhalādikam ।।

sarpa-lūtādi-daṃṣṭrāsu dāruṇaṃ jaṅgamaṃ viṣam ।
sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ ceti viṣaṃ proktam a-kṛtrimam ।।

kṛtrimaṃ gara-saṃjñaṃ tu kriyate vividhauṣadhaiḥ ।
hanti yoga-vaśenāśu cirāc cira-tarāc ca tat ।।

śopha-pāṇḍūdaronmāda-dur-nāmādīn karoti vā ।
tīkṣṇoṣṇa-rūkṣa-viśadaṃ vyavāyy āśu-karaṃ laghu ।।

-dur-nāmādīn karoti ca
vikāṣi sūkṣmam a-vyakta-rasaṃ viṣama-pāki ca ।
ojaso viparītaṃ tat tīkṣṇādyair anvitaṃ guṇaiḥ ।।

ikāśi sūkṣmam a-vyakta- ikāsi sūkṣmam a-vyakta- -rasair yuktam a-pāki ca 
jaso viparītaṃ tu
vāta-pittottaraṃ nṝṇāṃ sadyo harati jīvitam ।
viṣaṃ hi dehaṃ saṃprāpya prāg dūṣayati śoṇitam ।।

kapha-pittānilāṃś cānu samaṃ doṣān sahāśayān ।
tato hṛdayam āsthāya dehocchedāya kalpate ।।

ama-doṣaṃ sahāśayān amaṃ doṣān sahāya-vat ama-doṣaṃ sahāya-vat 
ama-doṣaṃ sahāśrayam eha-cchedāya kalpate
sthāvarasyopayuktasya vege pūrve prajāyate ।
jihvāyāḥ śyāva-tā stambho mūrchā trāsaḥ klamo vamiḥ ।।

egaḥ pūrvaṃ prajāyate ege pūrve ca jāyate
dvitīye vepathuḥ svedo dāhaḥ kaṇṭhe ca vedanā ।
viṣaṃ cāmāśayaṃ prāptaṃ kurute hṛdi vedanām ।।

tālu-śoṣas tṛtīye tu śūlaṃ cāmāśaye bhṛśam ।
dur-bale harite śūne jāyete cāsya locane ।।

ur-varṇe harite śūne ur-varṇe harite śūnye
pakvāśaya-gate toda-hidhmā-kāsāntra-kūjanam ।
caturthe jāyate vege śirasaś cāti-gauravam ।।

akvāśaya-gate todo idhmā kāsāntra-kūjanam
kapha-praseko vaivarṇyaṃ parva-bhedaś ca pañcame ।
sarva-doṣa-prakopaś ca pakvādhāne ca vedanā ।।

ṣaṣṭhe saṃjñā-praṇāśaś ca su-bhṛśaṃ cātisāryate ।
skandha-pṛṣṭha-kaṭī-bhaṅgo bhaven mṛtyuś ca saptame ।।

prathame viṣa-vege tu vāntaṃ śītāmbu-secinam ।
sarpir-madhubhyāṃ saṃyuktam a-gadaṃ pāyayed drutam ।।

rathame viṣa-vege atha
dvitīye pūrva-vad vāntaṃ viriktaṃ cānupāyayet ।
tṛtīye a-gada-pānaṃ tu hitaṃ nasyaṃ tathāñjanam ।।

caturthe sneha-saṃyuktam a-gadaṃ pratiyojayet ।
pañcame madhuka-kvātha-mākṣikābhyāṃ yutaṃ hitam ।।

ṣaṣṭhe atīsāra-vad siddhir avapīḍaś tu saptame ।
mūrdhni kāka-padaṃ kṛtvā sāsṛg vā piśitaṃ kṣipet ।।

vapīḍaś ca saptame
kośātaky agnikaḥ pāṭhā sūryavally-amṛtābhayāḥ ।
śeluḥ śirīṣaḥ kiṇihī haridre kṣaudra-sāhvayā ।।

ūryavally amṛtābhayā aridre kṣaudra-sāhvayam
punarnave tri-kaṭukaṃ bṛhatyau śārive balā ।
eṣāṃ yavāgūṃ niryūhe śītāṃ sa-ghṛta-mākṣikām ।।

unarnavā tri-kaṭukaṃ ṛhatyau śārive bale
yuñjyād vegāntare sarva-viṣa-ghnīṃ kṛta-karmaṇaḥ ।
tad-van madhūka-madhuka-padma-kesara-candanaiḥ ।।

añjanaṃ tagaraṃ kuṣṭhaṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilā ।
phalinī tri-kaṭu spṛkkā nāgapuṣpaṃ sa-kesaram ।।

hareṇur madhukaṃ māṃsī rocanā kākamālikā ।
śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarja-rasaḥ śatāhvā kuṅkumaṃ balā ।।

ocanā kālamālikā ocanā kālamañjikā
tamāla-pattra-tālīśa-bhūrjośīra-niśā-dvayam ।
kanyopavāsinī snātā śukla-vāsā madhu-drutaiḥ ।।

amāla-pattraṃ tālīśaṃ hūrjośīraṃ niśā-dvayam 
śukla-vāsā madhu-plutaiḥ
dvi-jān abhyarcya taiḥ puṣye kalpayed a-gadottamam ।
vaidyaś cātra tadā mantraṃ prayatātmā paṭhed imam ।।

vi-jān abhyarcya puṣyarkṣe aidyaś cāśu tadā mantraṃ
namaḥ puruṣa-siṃhāya namo nārāyaṇāya ca ।
yathāsau nābhijānāti raṇe kṛṣṇa-parājayam ।।

aṇe kṛṣṇaḥ parājayam
etena satya-vākyena a-gado me prasidhyatu ।
namo vaiḍūryamāte hulu hulu rakṣa māṃ sarva-viṣebhyaḥ ।।

ulu kulu rakṣa māṃ sarva-viṣebhyaḥ gauri gāndhāri cāṇḍāli mātaṅgi svāhā piṣṭe ca dvitīyo mantraḥ ।।

auri gāndhāri caṇḍāli mātaṅgi svāhā harimāyi svāhā ।।

āritamāyi svāhā
a-śeṣa-viṣa-vetāla-graha-kārmaṇa-pāpmasu ।
maraka-vyādhi-dur-bhikṣa-yuddhāśani-bhayeṣu ca ।।

pāna-nasyāñjanālepa-maṇi-bandhādi-yojitaḥ ।
eṣa candrodayo nāma śānti-svasty-ayanaṃ param ।।

śāntiḥ svasty-ayanaṃ param vāsavo vṛtram avadhīt samāliptaḥ kilāmunā ।।

samālipto amunā kila
jīrṇaṃ viṣa-ghnauṣadhibhir hataṃ vā dāvāgni-vātātapa-śoṣitaṃ vā ।
sva-bhāvato vā na guṇaiḥ su-yuktaṃ dūṣī-viṣākhyāṃ viṣam abhyupaiti ।।

va-bhāvato vā su-guṇair na yuktaṃ va-bhāvato vā sva-guṇair na yuktaṃ 
ūṣī-viṣākhyaṃ viṣam abhyupaiti
vīryālpa-bhāvād a-vibhāvyam etat kaphāvṛtaṃ varṣa-gaṇānubandhi ।
tenārdito bhinna-purīṣa-varṇo duṣṭāsra-rogī tṛḍ-a-rocakārtaḥ ।।

mūrchan vaman gadgada-vāg vimuhyan bhavec ca dūṣyodara-liṅga-juṣṭaḥ ।
āmāśaya-sthe kapha-vāta-rogī pakvāśaya-sthe anila-pitta-rogī ।।

bhaven naro dhvasta-śiro-ruhāṅgo vilūna-pakṣaḥ sa yathā vihaṅgaḥ ।
sthitaṃ rasādiṣv atha-vā vicitrān karoti dhātu-prabhavān vikārān ।।

prāg-vātā-jīrṇa-śītābhra-divā-svapnā-hitāśanaiḥ ।
duṣṭaṃ dūṣayate dhātūn ato dūṣī-viṣaṃ smṛtam ।।

uṣṭaṃ dūṣayate dhātuṃ ato dūṣī-viṣaṃ smṛtam
dūṣī-viṣārtaṃ su-svinnam ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca śodhitam ।
dūṣī-viṣārim a-gadaṃ lehayen madhunāplutam ।।

pippalyo dhyāmakaṃ māṃsī lodhram elā suvarcikā ।
kuṭannaṭaṃ nataṃ kuṣṭhaṃ yaṣṭī candana-gairikam ।।

dūṣī-viṣārir nāmnāyaṃ na cānya-trāpi vāryate ।
viṣa-digdhena viddhas tu pratāmyati muhur muhuḥ ।।

vi-varṇa-bhāvaṃ bhajate viṣādaṃ cāśu gacchati ।
kīṭair ivāvṛtaṃ cāsya gātraṃ cimicimāyate ।।

śroṇi-pṛṣṭha-śiraḥ-skandha-saṃdhayaḥ syuḥ sa-vedanāḥ ।
kṛṣṇa-duṣṭāsra-visrāvī tṛṇ-mūrchā-jvara-dāha-vān ।।

dṛṣṭi-kāluṣya-vamathu-śvāsa-kāsa-karaḥ kṣaṇāt ।
ā-rakta-pīta-pary-antaḥ śyāva-madhyo ati-rug vraṇaḥ ।।

śūyate pacyate sadyo gatvā māṃsaṃ ca kṛṣṇa-tām ।
praklinnaṃ śīryate abhīkṣṇaṃ sa-picchila-parisravam ।।

kuryād a-marma-viddhasya hṛdayāvaraṇaṃ drutam ।
śalyam ākṛṣya taptena lohenānu dahed vraṇam ।।

atha-vā muṣkaka-śvetā-soma-tvak-tāmravallitaḥ ।
śirīṣād gṛdhranakhyāś ca kṣāreṇa pratisārayet ।।

śukanāsā-prativiṣā-vyāghrī-mūlaiś ca lepayet ।
kīṭa-daṣṭa-cikitsāṃ ca kuryāt tasya yathārhataḥ ।।

vraṇe tu pūti-piśite kriyā pitta-visarpa-vat ।
saubhāgyārthaṃ striyo bhartre rājñe vā-rati-coditāḥ ।।

ājñe cā-rati-coditāḥ
garam āhāra-saṃpṛktaṃ yacchanty āsanna-vartinaḥ ।
nānā-prāṇy-aṅga-śamala-viruddhauṣadhi-bhasmanām ।।

ānā-prāṇy-aṅga-sa-mala-
viṣāṇāṃ cālpa-vīryāṇāṃ yogo gara iti smṛtaḥ ।
tena pāṇduḥ kṛśo alpāgniḥ kāsa-śvāsa-jvarārditaḥ ।।

iṣāṇāṃ manda-vīryāṇāṃ
vāyunā pratilomena svapna-cintā-parāyaṇaḥ ।
mahodara-yakṛt-plīhī dīna-vāg dur-balo alasaḥ ।।

ehodara-yakṛt-plīhī īna-vāg dur-balo alasaḥ
śopha-vān satatādhmātaḥ śuṣka-pāda-karaḥ kṣayī ।
svapne gomāyu-mārjāra-nakula-vyāla-vānarān ।।

prāyaḥ paśyati śuṣkāṃś ca vanaspati-jalāśayān ।
manyate kṛṣṇam ātmānaṃ gauro gauraṃ ca kālakaḥ ।।

vi-karṇa-nāsā-nayanaṃ paśyet tad-vihatendriyaḥ ।
etair anyaiś ca bahubhiḥ kliṣṭo ghorair upadravaiḥ ।।

aśyet tu vihatendriyaḥ
garārto nāśam āpnoti kaś-cit sadyo a-cikitsitaḥ ।
garārto vānta-vān bhuktvā tat pathyaṃ pāna-bhojanam ।।

śuddha-hṛc chīlayed dhema sūtra-sthāna-vidheḥ smaran ।
śarkarā-kṣaudra-saṃyuktaṃ cūrṇaṃ tāpya-suvarṇayoḥ ।।

ūtra-sthāna-vidhiṃ smaran
lehaḥ praśamayanty ugraṃ sarva-yoga-kṛtaṃ viṣam ।
mūrvāmṛtā-nata-kaṇā-paṭolī-cavya-citrakān ।।

vacā-musta-viḍaṅgāni takra-koṣṇāmbu-mastubhiḥ ।
pibed rasena vāmlena garopahata-pāvakaḥ ।।

ibed rasena cāmlena
pārāvatāmiṣa-śaṭhī-puṣkarāhva-śṛtaṃ himam ।
gara-tṛṣṇā-rujā-kāsa-śvāsa-hidhmā-jvarāpaham ।।

-puṣkarāhvaṃ śṛtaṃ himam
try-ūṣaṇaṃ pañca-lavaṇaṃ mañjiṣṭhāṃ rajanī-dvayam ।
sūkṣmailāṃ trivṛtāṃ pattraṃ viḍaṅgānīndravāruṇīm ।।

madhukaṃ ceti sa-kṣaudraṃ go-viṣāṇe nidhāpayet ।
tasmād uṣṇāmbunā mātrāṃ prāg-bhaktaṃ yojayet tathā ।।

viṣaṃ bhuktaṃ jarāṃ yāti nir-viṣe api na doṣa-kṛt ।
lākṣā-priyaṅgu-mañjiṣṭhāḥ sa-mṛṇāla-hareṇukāḥ ।।

sa-yaṣṭy-āhvā madhu-yutā basta-pittena kalpitāḥ ।
nikhaned go-viṣāṇa-sthāḥ sapta-rātraṃ mahī-tale ।।

tatra kṛtvā maṇiṃ hemnā baddhaṃ hastena dhārayet ।
saṃspṛṣṭaṃ sa-viṣaṃ tena sadyo bhavati nir-viṣam ।।

viṣa-prakṛti-kālānna-doṣa-dūṣyādi-saṃgame ।
viṣa-saṃkaṭam uddiṣṭaṃ śatasyaiko atra jīvati ।।

kṣut-tṛṣṇā-gharma-daurbalya-krodha-śoka-bhaya-śramaiḥ ।
a-jīrṇa-varco-drava-tā-pitta-māruta-vṛddhibhiḥ ।।

tila-puṣpa-phalāghrāṇa-bhū-bāṣpa-ghana-garjitaiḥ ।
hasti-mūṣika-vāditra-niḥsvanair viṣa-saṃkaṭaiḥ ।।

-bhū-bāṣpa-ghana-garjanaiḥ
puro-vātotpalāmoda-madanair vardhate viṣam ।
varṣāsu cāmbu-yoni-tvāt saṃkledaṃ guḍa-vad gatam ।।

arṣāsu vāmbu-yoni-tvāt
visarpati ghanāpāye tad agastyo hinasti ca ।
prayāti manda-vīrya-tvaṃ viṣaṃ tasmād ghanātyaye ।।

iti prakṛti-sātmyartu-sthāna-vega-balā-balam ।
ālocya nipuṇaṃ buddhyā karmān-antaram ācaret ।।

ślaiṣmikaṃ vamanair uṣṇa-rūkṣa-tīkṣṇaiḥ pralepanaiḥ ।
kaṣāya-kaṭu-tiktaiś ca bhojanaiḥ śamayed viṣam ।।

paittikaṃ sraṃsanaiḥ seka-pradehair bhṛśa-śītalaiḥ ।
kaṣāya-tikta-madhurair ghṛta-yuktaiś ca bhojanaiḥ ।।

vātātmakaṃ jayet svādu-snigdhāmla-lavaṇānvitaiḥ ।
sa-ghṛtair bhojanair lepais tathaiva piśitāśanaiḥ ।।

-snigdhāmla-lavaṇāyutaiḥ
nā-ghṛtaṃ sraṃsanaṃ śastaṃ pralepo bhojyam auṣadham ।
sarveṣu sarvāvasthāsu viṣeṣu na ghṛtopamam ।।

vidyate bheṣajaṃ kiñ-cid viśeṣāt prabale anile ।
a-yatnāc chleṣma-gaṃ sādhyaṃ yatnāt pittāśayāśrayam ।।

-yatnāc chlaiṣmikaṃ sādhyaṃ -yatnāc chleṣmakaṃ sādhyaṃ
atnāt pittāśayāśritam
su-duḥ-sādhyam a-sādhyaṃ vā vātāśaya-gataṃ viṣam ।।

jatu-sarja-rasośīra-sarṣapā-pattra-vālakaiḥ ।
sa-vaillāruṣkara-puraiḥ kusumair arjunasya ca ।।

ū̆ a-vailla-puṣkara-puraiḥ
dhūpo vāsa-gṛhe hanti viṣaṃ sthāvara-jaṅgamam ।
na tatra kīṭāḥ sa-viṣā nondurā na sarīsṛpāḥ ।।
na kṛtyāḥ kārmaṇādyāś ca dhūpo ayaṃ yatra dahyate ।।
uttarasthāna
darvī-karā maṇḍalino rājī-mantaś ca pannagāḥ ।
tri-dhā samāsato bhaumā bhidyante te tv aneka-dhā ।।

vyāsato yoni-bhedena nocyante an-upayoginaḥ ।
viśeṣād rūkṣa-kaṭukam amloṣṇaṃ svādu-śītalam ।।

ocyante an-upayogataḥ
viṣaṃ darvī-karādīnāṃ kramād vātādi-kopanam ।
tāruṇya-madhya-vṛddha-tve vṛṣṭi-śītātapeṣu ca ।।

viṣolbaṇā bhavanty ete vyantarā ṛtu-saṃdhiṣu ।
rathāṅga-lāṅgala-cchattra-svastikāṅkuśa-dhāriṇaḥ ।।

phaṇinaḥ śīghra-gatayaḥ sarpā darvī-karāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
jñeyā maṇḍalino a-bhogā maṇḍalair vividhaiś citāḥ ।।

arpā darvī-karā matāḥ
prāṃśavo manda-gamanā rājī-mantas tu rājibhiḥ ।
snigdhā vicitra-varṇābhis tiryag ūrdhvaṃ ca citritāḥ ।।

ājī-mantaś ca rājibhiḥ nigdhābhir bahu-varṇābhis
godhā-sutas tu gaudhero viṣe darvī-karaiḥ samaḥ ।
catuṣ-pād vyantarān vidyād eteṣām eva saṃkarāt ।।

odhā-sutas tu gaudheyo
vyāmiśra-lakṣaṇās te hi saṃnipāta-prakopaṇāḥ ।
āhārārthaṃ bhayāt pāda-sparśād ati-viṣāt krudhaḥ ।।

pāpa-vṛtti-tayā vairād devarṣi-yama-codanāt ।
daśanti sarpās teṣūktaṃ viṣādhikyaṃ yathottaram ।।

āpa-vṛtta-tayā vairād evarṣi-yama-nodanāt
ādiṣṭāt kāraṇaṃ jñātvā pratikuryād yathā-yatham ।
vyantaraḥ pāpa-śīla-tvān mārgam āśritya tiṣṭhati ।।

āviṣṭāt kāraṇaṃ jñātvā ārgam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
yatra lālā-parikleda-mātraṃ gātre pradṛśyate ।
na tu daṃṣṭrā-kṛtaṃ daṃśaṃ tat tuṇḍāhatam ādiśet ।।

-mātraṃ gātreṣu dṛśyate a tu daṃṣṭrā-kṣataṃ daṃśaṃ a tu daṃṣṭrā-kṣataṃ daṃśe 
aṃ tuṇḍāhataṃ ādiśet
ekaṃ daṃṣṭrā-padaṃ dve vā vyālīḍhākhyam a-śoṇitam ।
daṃṣṭrā-pade sa-rakte dve vyāluptaṃ trīṇi tāni tu ।।

yāluptaṃ trīṇi tāni ca
māṃsa-cchedād a-vicchinna-rakta-vāhīni daṣṭakam ।
daṃṣṭrā-padāni catvāri tad-vad daṣṭa-nipīḍitam ।।

nir-viṣaṃ dvayam atrādyam a-sādhyaṃ paścimaṃ vadet ।
viṣaṃ nāheyam a-prāpya raktaṃ dūṣayate vapuḥ ।।

raktam aṇv api tu prāptaṃ vardhate tailam ambu-vat ।
bhīros tu sarpa-saṃsparśād bhayena kupito anilaḥ ।।

aktam aṇv api tat prāptaṃ ardhate taila-bindu-vat
kadā-cit kurute śophaṃ sarpāṅgābhihataṃ tu tat ।
dur-gāndha-kāre viddhasya kena-cid daṣṭa-śaṅkayā ।।

ur-ge andhakāre viddhasya
viṣodvego jvaraś chardir mūrchā dāho api vā bhavet ।
glānir moho atisāro vā tac chaṅkā-viṣam ucyate ।।

iṣa-vegāj jvaraś chardir iṣodreko jvaraś chardir 
viṣodvegāj jvaraś chardir
tudyate sa-viṣo daṃśaḥ kaṇḍū-śopha-rujānvitaḥ ।
dahyate grathitaḥ kiñ-cid viparītas tu nir-viṣaḥ ।।

udyate viṣa-jo daṃśaḥ
pūrve darvī-kṛtāṃ vege duṣṭaṃ śyāvī-bhavaty asṛk ।
śyāva-tā tena vaktrādau sarpantīva ca kīṭakāḥ ।।

uṣṭaṃ śyāvaṃ bhavaty asṛk śyāva-tā netra-vaktrādau
dvitīye granthayo vege tṛtīye mūrdhni gauravam ।
dṛg-rodho daṃśa-vikledaś caturthe ṣṭhīvanaṃ vamiḥ ।।

ṛtīye mūrdha-gauravam ṛg-bādhā daṃśa-vikledaś 
caturthe ṣṭhevanaṃ vamiḥ
saṃdhi-viśleṣaṇaṃ tandrā pañcame parva-bhedanam ।
dāho hidhmā ca ṣaṣṭhe tu hṛt-pīḍā gātra-gauravam ।।

āho hidhmā ca ṣaṣṭhe ca
mūrchā-vipāko atīsāraḥ prāpya śukraṃ tu saptame ।
skandha-pṛṣṭha-kaṭī-bhaṅgaḥ sarva-ceṣṭā-nivartanam ।।

rāpya śukraṃ ca saptame
atha maṇḍali-daṣṭasya duṣṭaṃ pītī-bhavaty asṛk ।
tena pītāṅga-tā dāho dvitīye śvayathūdbhavaḥ ।।

uṣṭaṃ pītaṃ bhavaty asṛk
tṛtīye daṃśa-vikledaḥ svedas tṛṣṇā ca jāyate ।
caturthe jvaryate dāhaḥ pañcame sarva-gātra-gaḥ ।।

vedas tṛṣṇā prajāyate
daṣṭasya rājilair duṣṭaṃ pāṇḍu-tāṃ yāti śoṇitam ।
pāṇḍu-tā tena gātrāṇāṃ dvitīye guru-tāti ca ।।

tṛtīye daṃśa-vikledo nāsikākṣi-mukha-sravāḥ ।
caturthe garimā mūrdhno manyā-stambhaś ca pañcame ।।

gātra-bhaṅgo jvaraḥ śītaḥ śeṣayoḥ pūrva-vad vadet ।
kuryāt pañcasu vegeṣu cikitsāṃ na tataḥ param ।।

śeṣayoḥ pūrva-vad bhavet
jalāplutā rati-kṣīṇā bhītā nakula-nirjitāḥ ।
śīta-vātātapa-vyādhi-kṣut-tṛṣṇā-śrama-pīḍitāḥ ।।

tūrṇaṃ deśāntarāyātā vimukta-viṣa-kañcukāḥ ।
kuśauṣadhi-kaṇṭaka-vad ye caranti ca kānanam ।।

deśaṃ ca divyādhyuṣitaṃ sarpās te alpa-viṣā matāḥ ।
śmaśāna-citi-caityādau pañcamī-pakṣa-saṃdhiṣu ।।

eśaṃ ca vidyādhyuṣitaṃ
aṣṭamī-navamī-saṃdhyā-madhya-rātri-dineṣu ca ।
yāmyāgneya-maghāśleṣā-viśākhā-pūrva-nairṛte ।।

nairṛtākhye muhūrte ca daṣṭaṃ marmasu ca tyajet ।
daṣṭa-mātraḥ sitāsyākṣaḥ śīryamāṇa-śiro-ruhaḥ ।।

aṣṭa-mātras tu tāmrākṣaḥ
stabdha-jihvo muhur mūrchan śītocchvāso na jīvati ।
hidhmā śvāso vamiḥ kāso daṣṭa-mātrasya dehinaḥ ।।

śītocchvāsī na jīvati
jāyante yuga-pad yasya sa hṛc-chūlī na jīvati ।
phenaṃ vamati niḥ-saṃjñaḥ śyāva-pāda-karānanaḥ ।।

nāsāvasādo bhaṅgo aṅge viḍ-bhedaḥ ślatha-saṃdhi-tā ।
viṣa-pītasya daṣṭasya digdhenābhihatasya ca ।।

āsāvasādo ruk vāṅge
bhavanty etāni rūpāṇi saṃprāpte jīvita-kṣaye ।
na nasyaiś cetanā tīkṣṇair na kṣatāt kṣata-jāgamaḥ ।।

rāpte jīvita-saṃkṣaye
daṇḍāhatasya no rājī prayātasya yamāntikam ।
ato anya-thā tu tvarayā pradīptāgāra-vad bhiṣak ।।

rayāti sa yamāntikam
rakṣan kaṇṭha-gatān prāṇān viṣam āśu śamaṃ nayet ।
mātrā-śataṃ viṣaṃ sthitvā daṃśe daṣṭasya dehinaḥ ।।

dehaṃ prakramate dhātūn rudhirādīn pradūṣayan ।
etasminn antare karma daṃśasyotkartanādikam ।।

udhirādīn pradūṣayet
kuryac chīghraṃ yathā dehe viṣa-vallī na rohati ।
daṣṭa-mātro daśed āśu tam eva pavanāśinam ।।

am eva pavanāśanam
loṣṭaṃ mahīṃ vā daśanaiś chittvā cānu sa-saṃbhramam ।
niṣṭhīvena samālimped daṃśaṃ karṇa-malena vā ।।

hittvā cāśu sa-saṃbhramam
daṃśasyopari badhnīyād ariṣṭāṃ catur-aṅgule ।
kṣaumādibhir veṇikayā siddhair mantraiś ca mantra-vit ।।

ambu-vat setu-bandhena bandhena stabhyate viṣam ।
na vahanti sirāś cāsya viṣaṃ bandhābhipīḍitāḥ ।।

a vahanti sirās tasya iṣaṃ bandhana-pīḍitāḥ
niṣpīḍyānūddhared daṃśaṃ marma-saṃdhy-a-gataṃ tathā ।
na jāyate viṣād vego bīja-nāśād ivāṅkuraḥ ।।

iṣpīḍya coddhared daṃśaṃ a jāyate viṣāvego
daṃśaṃ maṇḍalināṃ muktvā pittala-tvād athāparam ।
prataptair hema-lohādyair dahed āśūlmukena vā ।।

karoti bhasma-sāt sadyo vahniḥ kiṃ nāma tu kṣatam ।
ācūṣet pūrṇa-vaktro vā mṛd-bhasmā-gada-go-mayaiḥ ।।

ahniḥ kiṃ nāma na kṣaṇāt ahniḥ kiṃ nāma na kṣaṇam
pracchāyāntar ariṣṭāyāṃ māṃsalaṃ tu viśeṣataḥ ।
aṅgaṃ sahaiva daṃśena lepayed a-gadair muhuḥ ।।

candanośīra-yuktena salilena ca secayet ।
viṣe pravisṛte vidhyet sirāṃ sā paramā kriyā ।।

rakte nirhriyamāṇe hi kṛtsnaṃ nirhriyate viṣam ।
dur-gandhaṃ sa-viṣaṃ raktam agnau caṭacaṭāyate ।।

ur-gandhi sa-viṣaṃ raktam
yathā-doṣaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca pūrva-val lakṣayed asṛk ।
sirāsv a-dṛśyamānāsu yojyāḥ śṛṅga-jalaukasaḥ ।।

śoṇitaṃ sruta-śeṣaṃ ca pravilīnaṃ viṣoṣmaṇā ।
lepa-sekaiḥ su-bahu-śaḥ stambhayed bhṛśa-śītalaiḥ ।।

a-skanne viṣa-vegād dhi mūrchāya-mada-hṛd-dravāḥ ।
bhavanti tān jayec chītair vījec cā-roma-harṣataḥ ।।

ījayed roma-harṣataḥ
skanne tu rudhire sadyo viṣa-vegaḥ praśāmyati ।
viṣaṃ karṣati tīkṣṇa-tvād dhṛdayaṃ tasya guptaye ।।

pibed ghṛtaṃ ghṛta-kṣaudram a-gadaṃ vā ghṛtāplutam ।
hṛdayāvaraṇe cāsya śleṣmā hṛdy upacīyate ।।

ṛdayāvaraṇenāsya
pravṛtta-gauravotkleśa-hṛl-lāsaṃ vāmayet tataḥ ।
dravaiḥ kāñjika-kaulattha-taila-madyādi-varjitaiḥ ।।

vamanair viṣa-hṛdbhiś ca naivaṃ vyāpnoti tad vapuḥ ।
bhujaṅga-doṣa-prakṛti-sthāna-vega-viśeṣataḥ ।।

su-sūkṣmaṃ samyag ālocya viśiṣṭāṃ cācaret kriyām ।
sindhuvārita-mūlāni śvetā ca girikarṇikā ।।

iśiṣṭāṃ vācaret kriyām
pānaṃ darvī-karair daṣṭe nasyaṃ madhu sa-pākalam ।
kṛṣṇa-sarpeṇa daṣṭasya limped daṃśaṃ hṛte asṛji ।।

asyaṃ sa-madhu pākalam asyaṃ sa-madhu vālakam 
asyaṃ madhu sa-vālakam
cāraṭī-nākulībhyāṃ vā tīkṣṇa-mūla-viṣeṇa vā ।
pānaṃ ca kṣaudra-mañjiṣṭhā-gṛha-dhūma-yutaṃ ghṛtam ।।

āne ca kṣaudra-mañjiṣṭhā-
taṇḍulīyaka-kāśmarya-kiṇihī-girikarṇikāḥ ।
mātuluṅgī sitā śeluḥ pāna-nasyāñjanair hitaḥ ।।

ātuluṅgaiḥ śiphā śeluḥ
a-gadaḥ phaṇināṃ ghore viṣe rājī-matām api ।
samāḥ sugandhā-mṛdvīkā-śvetākhyā-gajadantikāḥ ।।

amāḥ sugandhā mṛdvīkā śvetākhyā gajamṛttikā 
śvetākhyā gajavṛttikā
ardhāṃśaṃ saurasaṃ pattraṃ kapitthaṃ bilva-dāḍimam ।
sa-kṣaudro maṇḍali-viṣe viśeṣād a-gado hitaḥ ।।

pañca-valka-varā-yaṣṭī-nāgapuṣpailavālukam ।
jīvakarṣabhakau śītaṃ sitā padmakam utpalam ।।

añca-valka-balā-yaṣṭī- añca-valka-vacā-yaṣṭī- 
jīvakarṣabhakośīraṃ
sa-kṣaudro himavān nāma hanti maṇḍalināṃ viṣam ।
lepāc chvayathu-vīsarpa-visphoṭa-jvara-dāha-hā ।।

kāśmaryaṃ vaṭa-śuṅgāni jīvakarṣabhakau sitā ।
mañjiṣṭhā madhukaṃ ceti daṣṭo maṇḍalinā pibet ।।

āśmaryaṃ vaṭa-śṛṅgāni
vaṃśa-tvag-bīja-kaṭukā-pāṭalī-bīja-nāgaram ।
śirīṣa-bījātiviṣe mūlaṃ gāvedhukaṃ vacā ।।

-pāṭalā-bīja-nāgaram ūlaṃ gāvedhukaṃ vacām 
mūlaṃ śrīveṣṭakaṃ vacām
piṣṭo go-vāriṇāṣṭāṅgo hanti gonasa-jaṃ viṣam ।
kaṭukātiviṣā-kuṣṭha-gṛha-dhūma-hareṇukāḥ ।।

sa-kṣaudra-vyoṣa-tagarā ghnanti rājī-matāṃ viṣam ।
nikhanet kāṇḍa-citrāyā daṃśaṃ yāma-dvayaṃ bhuvi ।।

uddhṛtya pracchitaṃ sarpir-dhānya-mṛdbhyāṃ pralepayet ।
pibet purāṇaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ varā-cūrṇāvacūrṇitam ।।

ddhṛtya prasthitaṃ sarpir- arā-cūrṇa-vicūrṇitam
jīrṇe virikto bhuñjīta yavānnaṃ sūpa-saṃskṛtam ।
karavīrārka-kusuma-mūla-lāṅgalikā-kaṇāḥ ।।

īrṇe virikte bhuñjīta -mūlaṃ lāṅgalikā kaṇā
kalkayed āranālena pāṭhā-marica-saṃyutāḥ ।
eṣa vyantara-daṣṭānām a-gadaḥ sārvakārmikaḥ ।।

śirīṣa-puṣpa-sva-rase saptāhvaṃ maricaṃ sitam ।
bhāvitaṃ sarpa-daṣṭānāṃ pāna-nasyāñjane hitam ।।

āna-nasyāñjanair hitam āne nasye añjane hitam
dvi-palaṃ nata-kuṣṭhābhyāṃ ghṛta-kṣaudraṃ catuḥ-palam ।
api takṣaka-daṣṭānāṃ pānam etat sukha-pradam ।।

hṛta-kṣaudra-catuḥ-palam pi tārkṣaka-daṣṭānāṃ
atha darvī-kṛtāṃ vege pūrve visrāvya śoṇitam ।
a-gadaṃ madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ saṃyuktaṃ tvaritaṃ pibet ।।

dvitīye vamanaṃ kṛtvā tad-vad evā-gadaṃ pibet ।
viṣāpahe prayuñjīta tṛtīye añjana-nāvane ।।

iṣāpahaiḥ prayuñjīta
pibec caturthe pūrvoktāṃ yavāgūṃ vamane kṛte ।
ṣaṣṭha-pañcamayoḥ śītair digdhaṃ siktam abhīkṣṇa-śaḥ ।।

pāyayed vamanaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ yavāgūṃ ca viṣāpahaiḥ ।
a-gadaṃ saptame tīkṣṇaṃ yuñjyād añjana-nasyayoḥ ।।

kṛtvāvagāḍhaṃ śastreṇa mūrdhni kāka-padaṃ tataḥ ।
māṃsaṃ sa-rudhiraṃ tasya carma vā tatra nikṣipet ।।

tṛtīye vamitaḥ peyāṃ vege maṇḍalināṃ pibet ।
a-tīkṣṇam a-gadaṃ ṣaṣṭhe gaṇaṃ vā padmakādikam ।।

ṛtīye vāmitaḥ peyāṃ
ādye avagāḍhaṃ pracchāya vege daṣṭasya rājilaiḥ ।
alābunā hared raktaṃ pūrva-vac cā-gadaṃ pibet ।।

ṣaṣṭhe añjanaṃ tīkṣṇa-tamam avapīḍaṃ ca yojayet ।
an-ukteṣu ca vegeṣu kriyāṃ darvī-karoditām ।।

garbhiṇī-bāla-vṛddheṣu mṛduṃ vidhyet sirāṃ na ca ।
tvaṅ manohvā niśe vakraṃ rasaḥ śārdūla-jo nakhaḥ ।।

urviṇī-bāla-vṛddheṣu ṛdu vidhyet sirāṃ na ca 
tvaṅ manohvā niśe vaktraṃ
tamālaḥ kesaraṃ śītaṃ pītaṃ taṇḍula-vāriṇā ।
hanti sarva-viṣāṇy etad vajraṃ vajram ivāsurān ।।

anti sarva-viṣāṇy etac hakra-vajram ivāsurān 
vajri-vajram ivāsurān
bilvasya mūlaṃ surasasya puṣpaṃ phalaṃ karañjasya nataṃ surāhvam ।
phala-trikaṃ vyoṣa-niśā-dvayaṃ ca bastasya mūtreṇa su-sūkṣma-piṣṭam ।।

hala-trayaṃ vyoṣa-niśā-dvayaṃ ca
bhujaṅga-lūtondura-vṛścikādyair viṣūcikā-jīrṇa-gara-jvaraiś ca ।
ārtān narān bhūta-vidharṣitāṃś ca svasthī-karoty añjana-pāna-nasyaiḥ ।।

ārtān narān bhūta-vimarditāṃś ca
pralepādyaiś ca niḥśeṣaṃ daṃśād apy uddhared viṣam ।
bhūyo vegāya jāyeta śeṣaṃ dūṣī-viṣāya vā ।।

śeṣaṃ dūṣī-viṣaṃ yathā śeṣaṃ dūṣī-viṣāya ca
viṣāpāye anilaṃ kruddhaṃ snehādibhir upācaret ।
taila-madya-kulatthāmla-varjyaiḥ pavana-nāśanaiḥ ।।

pittaṃ pitta-jvara-haraiḥ kaṣāya-sneha-vastibhiḥ ।
sa-mākṣikeṇa vargeṇa kapham āragvadhādinā ।।

sitā vaigandhiko drākṣā payasyā madhukaṃ madhu ।
pānaṃ sa-mantra-pūtāmbu prokṣaṇaṃ sāntva-harṣaṇam ।।

itā vaigandhako drākṣā
sarpāṅgābhihate yuñjyāt tathā śaṅkā-viṣārdite ।
karketanaṃ marakataṃ vajraṃ vāraṇa-mauktikam ।।

vaiḍūryaṃ gardabha-maṇiṃ picukaṃ viṣa-mūṣikām ।
himavad-giri-saṃbhūtāṃ somarājīṃ punarnavām ।।

aiḍūrya-gardabha-maṇiṃ icukaṃ viṣa-dūṣikām
tathā droṇāṃ mahā-droṇāṃ mānasīṃ sarpa-jaṃ maṇim ।
viṣāṇi viṣa-śānty-arthaṃ vīrya-vanti ca dhārayet ।।

athā droṇaṃ mahā-droṇaṃ
chattrī jharjhara-pāṇiś ca cared rātrau viśeṣataḥ ।
tac-chāyā-śabda-vitrastāḥ praṇaśyanti bhujaṅgamāḥ ।।

hattrī jarjara-pāṇiś ca hattrī jarjhara-pāṇiś ca hattrī jharjara-pāṇiś ca 
ared rātrau ca sarva-dā idravanti bhujaṅgamāḥ
vāri-guñjā-phalośīraṃ netrayor viṣa-duṣṭayoḥ ।
añjanaṃ vāriṇā piṣṭaṃ gāruḍaṃ garuḍopamam ।।

uttarasthāna
sarpāṇām eva viṇ-mūtra-śukrāṇḍa-śava-kotha-jāḥ ।
doṣair vyastaiḥ samastaiś ca yuktāḥ kīṭāś catur-vidhāḥ ।।

daṣṭasya kīṭair vāyavyair daṃśas toda-rujolbaṇaḥ ।
āgneyair alpa-saṃsrāvo dāha-rāga-visarpa-vān ।।

pakva-pīlu-phala-prakhyaḥ kharjūra-sadṛśo atha-vā ।
kaphādhikair manda-rujaḥ pakvodumbara-saṃnibhaḥ ।।

srāvāḍhyaḥ sarva-liṅgas tu vivarjyaḥ sāṃnipātikaiḥ ।
vegāś ca sarpa-vac chopho vardhiṣṇur visra-rakta-tā ।।

ivarjyaḥ sāṃnipātikaḥ
śiro-'kṣi-gauravaṃ mūrchā bhramaḥ śvāso ati-vedanā ।
sarveṣāṃ karṇikā śopho jvaraḥ kaṇḍūr a-rocakaḥ ।।

hramaḥ śvāso ati-vedanāḥ
vṛścikasya viṣaṃ tīkṣṇam ādau dahati vahni-vat ।
ūrdhvam ārohati kṣipraṃ daṃśe paścāt tu tiṣṭhati ।।

c daṃśe paścāc ca tiṣṭhati
daṃśaḥ sadyo ati-ruk śyāvas tudyate sphuṭatīva ca ।
te gavādi-śakṛt-kothād digdha-daṣṭādi-kothataḥ ।।

sarpa-kothāc ca saṃbhūtā manda-madhya-mahā-viṣāḥ ।
mandāḥ pītāḥ sitāḥ śyāvā rūkṣāḥ karbura-mecakāḥ ।।

ūkṣa-karbura-mecakāḥ
romaśā bahu-parvāṇo lohitāḥ pāṇḍurodarāḥ ।
dhūmrodarās tri-parvāṇo madhyās tu kapilāruṇāḥ ।।

piśaṅgāḥ śabarāś citrāḥ śoṇitābhā mahā-viṣāḥ ।
agny-ābhā dvy-eka-parvāṇo raktāsita-sitodarāḥ ।।

tair daṣṭaḥ śūna-rasanaḥ stabdha-gātro jvarārditaḥ ।
khair vamañ choṇitaṃ kṛṣṇam indriyārthān a-saṃvidan ।।

svidyan mūrchan viśuṣkāsyo vihvalo vedanāturaḥ ।
viśīryamāṇa-māṃsaś ca prāya-śo vijahāty asūn ।।

ucciṭiṅgas tu vaktreṇa daśaty abhyadhika-vyathaḥ ।
sādhyato vṛścikāt stambhaṃ śephaso hṛṣṭa-roma-tām ।।

cciṭaṅgas tu vaktreṇa o adhamo vṛścikāt stambhaṃ
karoti sekam aṅgānāṃ daṃśaḥ śītāmbuneva ca ।
uṣṭra-dhūmaḥ sa evokto rātri-cārāc ca rātrikaḥ ।।

aṃśe śītāmbuneva ca
vāta-pittottarāḥ kīṭāḥ ślaiṣmikāḥ kaṇabhondurāḥ ।
prāyo vātolbaṇa-viṣā vṛścikāḥ soṣṭra-dhūmakāḥ ।।

yasya yasyaiva doṣasya liṅgādhikyaṃ pratarkayet ।
tasya tasyauṣadhaiḥ kuryād viparīta-guṇaiḥ kriyām ।।

iṅgādhikyaṃ pravartayet
hṛt-pīḍordhvānila-stambhaḥ sirāyāmo asthi-parva-ruk ।
ghūrṇanodveṣṭanaṃ gātra-śyāva-tā vātike viṣe ।।

saṃjñā-nāśoṣṇa-niśvāsau hṛd-dāhaḥ kaṭukāsya-tā ।
māṃsāvadaraṇaṃ śopho rakta-pītaś ca paittike ।।

aktaḥ pītaś ca paittike
chardy-a-rocaka-hṛl-lāsa-prasekotkleśa-pīnasaiḥ ।
sa-śaitya-mukha-mādhuryair vidyāc chleṣmādhikaṃ viṣam ।।

piṇyākena vraṇālepas tailābhyaṅgaś ca vātike ।
svedo nāḍī-pulākādyair bṛṃhaṇaś ca vidhir hitaḥ ।।

paittikaṃ stambhayet sekaiḥ pradehaiś cāti-śītalaiḥ ।
lekhana-cchedana-sveda-vamanaiḥ ślaiṣmikaṃ jayet ।।

kīṭānāṃ tri-prakārāṇāṃ traividhyena kriyā hitā ।
svedālepana-sekāṃs tu koṣṇān prāyo avacārayet ।।

raividhyena kriyā hitāḥ avoṣṇān pravicārayet
anya-tra mūrchitād daṃśa-pākataḥ kothato atha-vā ।
nṛ-keśāḥ sarṣapāḥ pītā guḍo jīrṇaś ca dhūpanam ।।

viṣa-daṃśasya sarvasya kāśyapaḥ param abravīt ।
viṣa-ghnaṃ ca vidhiṃ sarvaṃ kuryāt saṃśodhanāni ca ।।

aśyapaḥ param abravīt
sādhayet sarpa-vad daṣṭān viṣograiḥ kīṭa-vṛścikaiḥ ।
taṇḍulīyaka-tulyāṃśāṃ trivṛtāṃ sarpiṣā pibet ।।

yāti kīṭa-viṣaiḥ kampaṃ na kailāsa ivānilaiḥ ।
kṣīri-vṛkṣa-tvag-ālepaḥ śuddhe kīṭa-viṣāpahaḥ ।।

muktā-lepo varaḥ śopha-toda-dāha-jvara-praṇut ।
vacā-hiṅgu-viḍaṅgāni saindhavaṃ gaja-pippalī ।।

pāṭhā prativiṣā vyoṣaṃ kāśyapena vinirmitam ।
daśāṅgam a-gadaṃ pītvā sarva-kīṭa-viṣaṃ jayet ।।

sadyo vṛścika-jaṃ daṃśaṃ cakra-tailena secayet ।
vidārigandhā-siddhena kavoṣṇenetareṇa vā ।।

lavaṇottama-yuktena sarpiṣā vā punaḥ punaḥ ।
siñcet koṣṇāranālena sa-kṣīra-lavaṇena vā ।।

a-kṣāra-lavaṇena vā
upanāho ghṛte bhṛṣṭaḥ kalko ajājyāḥ sa-saindhavaḥ ।
ādaṃśaṃ sveditaṃ cūrṇaiḥ pracchāya pratisārayet ।।

panāhe ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaḥ panāho ghṛta-bhṛṣṭaḥ
rajanī-saindhava-vyoṣa-śirīṣa-phala-puṣpa-jaiḥ ।
mātuluṅgāmla-go-mūtra-piṣṭaṃ ca surasāgra-jam ।।

ātuluṅgaṃ tu go-mūtra- -piṣṭaḥ sa-surasārjakaḥ
lepaḥ sukhoṣṇaś ca hitaḥ piṇyāko go-mayo api vā ।
pāne sarpir madhu-yutaṃ kṣīraṃ vā bhūri-śarkaram ।।

iṇyāko go-mayena vā
pārāvata-śakṛt pathyā tagaraṃ viśva-bheṣajam ।
bījapūra-rasonmiśraḥ paramo vṛścikā-gadaḥ ।।

aramo vṛścike a-gadaḥ aramo vṛściko a-gadaḥ
sa-śaivaloṣṭra-daṃṣṭrā ca hanti vṛścika-jaṃ viṣam ।
hiṅgunā haritālena mātuluṅga-rasena ca ।।

a-saindhavoṣṭra-daṃṣṭrā ca ātuluṅga-rasena vā
lepāñjanābhyāṃ guṭikā paramaṃ vṛścikāpahā ।
karañjārjuna-śelūnāṃ kaṭabhyāṃ kuṭajasya ca ।।

śirīṣasya ca puṣpāṇi mastunā daṃśa-lepanam ।
yo muhyati praśvasiti pralapaty ugra-vedanaḥ ।।

tasya pathyā-niśā-kṛṣṇā-mañjiṣṭhātiviṣoṣaṇam ।
sālābu-vṛntaṃ vārtāka-rasa-piṣṭaṃ pralepanam ।।

śalāṭu-vṛntaṃ vārtāka- sarva-tra cogrāli-viṣe pāyayed dadhi-sarpiṣī ।।
vidhyet sirāṃ vidadhyāc ca vamanāñjana-nāvanam ।।uṣṇa-snigdhāmla-madhuraṃ bhojanaṃ cānilāpaham ।।
nāgaraṃ gṛha-kapota-purīṣaṃ bījapūraka-raso haritālam ।
saindhavaṃ ca vinihanty a-gado ayaṃ lepato ali-kula-jaṃ viṣam āśu ।।

ante vṛścika-daṣṭānāṃ samudīrṇe bhṛśaṃ viṣe ।
viṣeṇālepayed daṃśam ucciṭiṅge apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।।

nāga-purīṣa-cchattraṃ rohiṣa-mūlaṃ ca śelu-toyena ।
kuryād guṭikāṃ lepād iyam ali-viṣa-nāśanī śreṣṭhā ।।

arkasya dugdhena śirīṣa-bījaṃ trir bhāvitaṃ pippali-cūrṇa-miśram ।
eṣo a-gado hanti viṣāṇi kīṭa-bhujaṅga-lūtondura-vṛścikānām ।।

śirīṣa-puṣpaṃ sa-karañja-bījaṃ kāśmīra-jaṃ kuṣṭha-manaḥśile ca ।
eṣo a-gado rātrika-vṛścikānāṃ saṃkrānti-kārī kathito jinena ।।

śirīṣa-bījaṃ sa-karañja-bījaṃ
kīṭebhyo dāruṇa-tarā lūṭāḥ ṣo-ḍaśa tā jaguḥ ।
aṣṭā-viṃśatir ity eke tato apy anye tu bhūyasīḥ ।।

sahasra-raśmy-anucarā vadanty anye sahasra-śaḥ ।
bahūpadrava-rūpā tu lūtaikaiva viṣātmikā ।।

rūpāṇi nāmatas tasyā dur-jñeyāny ati-saṃkarāt ।
nāsti sthāna-vyavasthā ca doṣato ataḥ pracakṣate ।।

kṛcchra-sādhyā pṛthag-doṣair a-sādhyā nicayena sā ।
tad-daṃśaḥ paittiko dāha-tṛṭ-sphoṭa-jvara-moha-vān ।।

bhṛśoṣṃā rakta-pītābhaḥ kledī drākṣā-phalopamaḥ ।
ślaiṣmikaḥ kaṭhinaḥ pāṇḍuḥ parūṣaka-phalākṛtiḥ ।।

hṛśoṣṃa-rakta-pītābhaḥ
nidrāṃ śīta-jvaraṃ kāsaṃ kaṇḍūṃ ca kurute bhṛśam ।
vātikaḥ paruṣaḥ śyāvaḥ parva-bheda-jvara-pradaḥ ।।

tad-vibhāgaṃ yathā-svaṃ ca doṣa-liṅgair vibhāvayet ।
a-sādhyāyāṃ tu hṛn-moha-śvāsa-hidhmā-śiro-grahāḥ ।।

-śvāsa-hidhmā-śiro-rujāḥ
śveta-pītāsitā-raktāḥ piṭikāḥ śvayathūdbhavaḥ ।
vepathur vamathur dāhas tṛḍ āndhyaṃ vakra-nāsa-tā ।।

śveta-pītāsitā-rakta- -piṭikā-śvayathūdbhavaḥ ṛḍ 
āndhyaṃ vakra-nāsikā
śyāvauṣṭha-vaktra-danta-tvaṃ pṛṣṭha-grīvāvabhañjanam ।
pakva-jambū-sa-varṇaṃ ca daṃśāt sravati śoṇitam ।।

sarvāpi sarva-jā prāyo vyapadeśas tu bhūyasā ।
tīkṣṇa-madhyāvara-tvena sā tri-dhā hanty upekṣitā ।।

ā tri-dhā hanty upekṣayā
saptāhena daśāhena pakṣeṇa ca paraṃ kramāt ।
lūtā-daṃśaś ca sarvo api dadrū-maṇḍala-saṃnibhaḥ ।।

ūtā-daṃśas tu sarvo api
sito asito aruṇaḥ pītaḥ śyāvo vā mṛdur unnataḥ ।
madhye kṛṣṇo atha-vā śyāvaḥ pary-ante jālakāvṛtaḥ ।।

itāsito aruṇaḥ pītaḥ
visarpa-vāṃś chopha-yutas tapyate bahu-vedanaḥ ।
jvarāśu-pāka-vikleda-kothāvadaraṇānvitaḥ ।।

kledena yat spṛśaty aṅgaṃ tatrāpi kurute vraṇam ।
śvāsa-daṃṣṭrā-śakṛn-mūtra-śukra-lālā-nakhārtavaiḥ ।।

aṣṭābhir udvamaty eṣā viṣaṃ vaktrād viśeṣataḥ ।
lūtā nābher daśaty ūrdhvam ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca kīṭakāḥ ।।

ṣṭābhir udvamanty etā iṣaṃ vaktrair viśeṣataḥ ūtā nābher daśanty ūrdhvam ūrdhvaṃ vādhaś ca kīṭakāḥ ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca kīṭakaḥ 
dhaś ca viṣa-kīṭakāḥ
tad-dūṣitaṃ ca vastrādi dehe pṛktaṃ vikāra-kṛt ।
dinārdhaṃ lakṣyate naiva daṃśo lūtā-viṣodbhavaḥ ।।

sūcī-vyadha-vad ābhāti tato asau prathame ahani ।
a-vyakta-varṇaḥ pracalaḥ kiñ-cit-kaṇḍū-rujānvitaḥ ।।

ūcī-viddha-vad ābhāti
dvitīye abhyunnato anteṣu piṭikair iva vācitaḥ ।
vyakta-varṇo nato madhye kaṇḍū-mān granthi-saṃnibhaḥ ।।

vitīye aty-unnato anteṣu iṭikair iva cācitaḥ
tṛtīye sa-jvaro roma-harṣa-kṛd rakta-maṇḍalaḥ ।
śarāva-rūpas todāḍhyo roma-kūpeṣu sāsravaḥ ।।

oma-kūpeṣu sa-sravaḥ
mahāṃś caturthe śvayathus tāpa-śvāsa-bhrama-pradaḥ ।
vikārān kurute tāṃs tān pañcame viṣa-kopa-jān ।।

ṣaṣṭhe vyāpnoti marmāṇi saptame hanti jīvitam ।
iti tīkṣṇaṃ viṣaṃ madhyaṃ hīnaṃ ca vibhajed ataḥ ।।

ṣaṣṭhe prāpnoti marmāṇi
eka-viṃśati-rātreṇa viṣaṃ śāmyati sarva-thā ।
athāśu lūtā-daṣṭasya śastreṇādaṃśam uddharet ।।

aṃśaṃ śastreṇa coddharet
dahec ca jāmbavauṣṭhādyair na tu pittottaraṃ dahet ।
karkaśaṃ bhinna-romāṇaṃ marma-saṃdhy-ādi-saṃśritam ।।

prasṛtaṃ sarvato daṃśaṃ na cchindīta dahen na ca ।
lepayed dagdham a-gadair madhu-saindhava-saṃyutaiḥ ।।

a cchindīta dahen na vā
su-śītaiḥ secayec cānu kaṣāyaiḥ kṣīri-vṛkṣa-jaiḥ ।
sarvato apahared raktaṃ śṛṅgādyaiḥ sirayāpi vā ।।

seka-lepās tataḥ śītā bodhi-śleṣmātakākṣakaiḥ ।
phalinī-dvi-niśā-kṣaudra-sarpirbhiḥ padmakāhvayaḥ ।।

ekālepās tataḥ śītā odhi-śleṣmātakākṣikaiḥ odhi-śleṣmātakākṣa-jaiḥ 
halinī-dvi-niśā-śreṣṭhā-
a-śeṣa-lūtā-kīṭānām a-gadaḥ sārvakārmikaḥ ।
haridrā-dvaya-pattaṅga-mañjiṣṭhā-nata-kesaraiḥ ।।

sa-kṣaudra-sarpiḥ pūrvasmād adhikaś campakāhvayaḥ ।
tad-vad go-maya-niṣpīḍa-śarkarā-ghṛta-mākṣikaiḥ ।।

ad-vad go-maya-niṣpīḍā-
apāmārga-mano'hvāla-dārvī-dhyāmaka-gairikaiḥ ।
natailā-kuṣṭha-marica-yaṣṭy-āhva-ghṛta-mākṣikaiḥ ।।

a-gado mandaro nāma tathānyo gandha-mādanaḥ ।
nata-lodhra-vacā-kaṭvī-pāṭhailā-pattra-kuṅkumaiḥ ।।

mañjiṣṭhā-śleṣmātaka-rajanī-suvahā-śirīṣa-pālindyaḥ ।
sa-sindhuvārā viṣaṃ ghnanti sailā-candana-kanakāḥ ।।

viṣa-ghnaṃ bahu-doṣeṣu prayuñjīta viśodhanam ।
yaṣṭy-āhva-madanāṅkolla-jālinī-sindhuvārikāḥ ।।

iṣa-ghnair bahu-doṣeṣu -jālinī-sindhuvāritān 
-jālinī-sindhuvāritam
kaphe jyeṣṭhāmbunā pītvā viṣam āśu samudvamet ।
śirīṣa-pattra-tvaṅ-mūla-phalaṃ vāṅkolla-mūla-vat ।।

-phalaṃ cāṅkolla-mūla-vat
virecayec ca tri-phalā-nīlinī-trivṛtādibhiḥ ।
nivṛtte dāha-śophādau karṇikāṃ pātayed vraṇāt ।।

-phalinī-trivṛtādibhiḥ
kusumbha-puṣpaṃ go-dantaḥ svarṇakṣīrī kapota-viṭ ।
trivṛtā saindhavaṃ dantī karṇikā-pātanaṃ tathā ।।

usumbha-puṣpa-go-danta- -svarṇakṣīrī-kapota-viṭ 
karṇikā-pātanaṃ param
mūlam uttaravāruṇyā vaṃśa-nirlekha-saṃyutam ।
tad-vac ca saindhavaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ dantī kaṭuka-daugdhikam ।।

rāja-kośātakī-mūlaṃ kiṇvo vā mathitodbhavaḥ ।
karṇikā-pāta-samaye bṛṃhayec ca viṣāpahaiḥ ।।

iṭṭo vā mathitodbhavaḥ iṇo vā mathitodbhavaḥ 
bṛṃhayeta viṣāpahaiḥ
sneha-kāryam a-śeṣaṃ ca sarpiṣaiva samācaret ।
viṣasya vṛddhaye tailam agner iva tṛṇolupam ।।

iṣam āvardhayet tailam gner iva tṛṇolapam
hrīvera-vaikaṅkata-gopakanyā-mustā-śamī-candana-ṭuṇṭukāni ।
śaivāla-nīlotpala-vakra-yaṣṭī-tvaṅ-nākulī-padmaka-rāṭha-madhyam ।।

-mustā-śamī-candana-tindukāni
rajanī-ghana-sarpalocanā-kaṇa-śuṇṭhī-kaṇa-mūla-citrakāḥ ।
varuṇāguru-bilva-pāṭalī-picumandāmaya-śelu-kesaram ।।

aruṇāguru-bilva-pāṭalā-
bilva-candana-natotpala-śuṇṭhī-pippalī-nicula-vetasa-kuṣṭham ।
śukti-śāka-vara-pāṭali-bhārgī-sindhuvāra-karaghāṭa-varāṅgam ।।

śukti-śābaraka-pāṭali-bhārgī- -sindhuvāra-karahāṭa-varāṅgam
pitta-kaphānila-lūtāḥ pānāñjana-nasya-lepa-sekena ।
a-gada-varā vṛtta-sthāḥ ku-gatīr iva vārayanty ete ।।

u-gatīr iva dārayanty ete u-matīr iva dārayanty ete 
u-matīr iva vārayanty ete
lodhraṃ sevyaṃ padmakaṃ padma-reṇuḥ kālīyākhyaṃ candanaṃ yac ca raktam ।
kāntā-puṣpaṃ dugdhinīkā mṛṇālaṃ lūtāḥ sarvā ghnanti sarva-kriyābhiḥ ।।

uttarasthāna
lālanaś capalaḥ putro hasiraś cikkiro ajiraḥ ।
kaṣāya-dantaḥ kulakaḥ kokilaḥ kapilo asitaḥ ।।

asiraś cikriro ajanaḥ asiraś cikkiro ajaraḥ asiraś cikilo 
ajiraḥ
aruṇaḥ śabaraḥ śvetaḥ kapotaḥ palitonduraḥ ।
chucchundaro rasālākhyo daśāṣṭau ceti mūṣikāḥ ।।

apotaḥ palitonduruḥ hucchundaro balāsākhyo hucchundaro rasālākṣo 
aśa cāṣṭau ca mūṣikāḥ
śukraṃ patati yatraiṣāṃ śukra-digdhaiḥ spṛśanti vā ।
yad aṅgam aṅgais tatrāsre dūṣite pāṇḍu-tāṃ gate ।।

granthayaḥ śvayathuḥ koṭho maṇḍalāni bhramo a-ruciḥ ।
śīta-jvaro ati-ruk sādo vepathuḥ parva-bhedanam ।।

ranthayaḥ śvayathuḥ kotho
roma-harṣaḥ srutir mūrchā dīrgha-kālānubandhanam ।
śleṣmānubaddha-bahv-ākhu-potaka-cchardanaṃ sa-tṛṭ ।।

śleṣmānubandha-bahv-ākhu- śleṣmānuviddha-bahv-ākhu- 
-potaka-cchardanaṃ sakṛt
vyavāyy ākhu-viṣaṃ kṛcchraṃ bhūyo bhūyaś ca kupyati ।
mūrchāṅga-śopha-vaivarṇya-kleda-śabdā-śruti-jvarāḥ ।।

śiro-guru-tvaṃ lālāsṛk-chardiś cā-sādhya-lakṣaṇam ।
śūna-vastiṃ vi-varṇauṣṭham ākhv-ābhair granthibhiś citam ।।

chucchundara-sa-gandhaṃ ca varjayed ākhu-dūṣitam ।
śunaḥ śleṣmolbaṇā doṣāḥ saṃjñāṃ saṃjñā-vahāśritāḥ ।।

muṣṇantaḥ kurvate kṣobhaṃ dhātūnām ati-dāruṇam ।
lālā-vān andha-badhiraḥ sarvataḥ so abhidhāvati ।।

srasta-puccha-hanu-skandhaḥ śiro-duḥkhī natānanaḥ ।
daṃśas tena vidaṣṭasya suptaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kṣaraty asṛk ।।

hṛc-chiro-rug-jvara-stambha-tṛṣṇā-mūrchodbhavo anu ca ।
anenānye api boddhavyā vyālā daṃṣṭrā-prahāriṇaḥ ।।

ṛc-chiro-rug-jvara-stambhas ṛc-chiro-rug jvaraḥ stambhas ṛṣṇā-mūrchodbhavo anu ca ṛṣṇā mūrchodbhavo anu ca 
yāla-daṃṣṭrā-prahāriṇaḥ
śṛgālāśvatarāśvarkṣa-dvīpi-vyāghra-vṛkādayaḥ ।
kaṇḍū-nistoda-vaivarṇya-supti-kleda-jvara-bhramāḥ ।।

vidāha-rāga-ruk-pāka-śopha-granthi-vikuñcanam ।
daṃśāvadaraṇaṃ sphoṭāḥ karṇikā maṇḍalāni ca ।।

sarva-tra sa-viṣe liṅgaṃ viparītaṃ tu nir-viṣe ।
daṣṭo yena tu tac-ceṣṭā-rutaṃ kurvan vinaśyati ।।

paśyaṃs tam eva cā-kasmād ādarśa-salilādiṣu ।
yo adbhyas trasyed a-daṣṭo api śabda-saṃsparśa-darśanaiḥ ।।

śabda-sparśa-nidarśanaiḥ
jala-saṃtrāsa-nāmānaṃ daṣṭaṃ tam api varjayet ।
ākhunā daṣṭa-mātrasya daṃśaṃ kāṇḍena dāhayet ।।

darpaṇenātha-vā tīvra-rujā syāt karṇikānya-thā ।
dagdhaṃ visrāvayed daṃśaṃ pracchitaṃ ca pralepayet ।।

agdhvā visrāvayed daṃśaṃ racchinnaṃ ca pralepayet
śirīṣa-rajanī-vakra-kuṅkumāmṛtavallibhiḥ ।
agāra-dhūma-mañjiṣṭhā-rajanī-lavaṇottamaiḥ ।।

lepo jayaty ākhu-viṣaṃ karṇikāyāś ca pātanaḥ ।
tato amlaiḥ kṣālayitvānu toyair anu ca lepayet ।।

iṣṭair anu ca lepayet
pālindī-śveta-kaṭabhī-bilva-mūla-guḍūcibhiḥ ।
anyaiś ca viṣa-śopha-ghnaiḥ sirāṃ vā mokṣayed drutam ।।

irāṃ vā mocayed drutam
chardanaṃ nīlinī-kvāthaiḥ śukākhyāṅkollayor api ।
kośātakyāḥ śukākhyāyāḥ phalaṃ jīmūtakasya ca ।।

ośavatyāḥ śukākhyāyāḥ
madanasya ca saṃcūrṇya dadhnā pītvā viṣaṃ vamet ।
vacā-madana-jīmūta-kuṣṭhaṃ vā mūtra-peṣitam ।।

pūrva-kalpena pātavyaṃ sarvondura-viṣāpaham ।
virecanaṃ trivṛn-nīlī-tri-phalā-kalka iṣyate ।।

irecane trivṛn-nīlī-
śiro-virecane sāraḥ śirīṣasya phalāni ca ।
añjanaṃ go-maya-raso vyoṣa-sūkṣma-rajo-'nvitaḥ ।।

ñjane go-maya-raso yoṣa-sūkṣma-rajo-'nvitaḥ
kapittha-go-maya-raso madhu-mān avalehanam ।
taṇḍulīyaka-mūlena siddhaṃ pāne hitaṃ ghṛtam ।।

adhu-mān avalehane
dvi-niśā-kaṭabhī-raktā-yaṣṭy-āhvair vāmṛtānvitaiḥ ।
āsphota-mūla-siddhaṃ vā pañca-kāpittham eva vā ।।

sindhuvāraṃ nataṃ śigru-bilva-mūlaṃ punarnavā ।
vacā-śvadaṃṣṭrā-jīmūtam eṣāṃ kvāthaṃ sa-mākṣikam ।।

indhuvāra-nataṃ śigru- -bilva-mūlaṃ punarnavam
pibec chāly-odanaṃ dadhnā bhuñjāno mūṣikārditaḥ ।
takreṇa śarapuṅkhāyā bījaṃ saṃcūrṇya vā pibet ।।

aṅkolla-mūla-kalko vā basta-mūtreṇa kalkitaḥ ।
pānālepanayor yuktaḥ sarvākhu-viṣa-nāśanaḥ ।।

āna-lepanayor yuktaḥ
kapittha-madhya-tilaka-tilāṅkolla-jaṭāḥ pibet ।
gavāṃ mūtreṇa payasā mañjarīṃ tilakasya vā ।।

apittha-madhya-tilakaṃ apittha-madhyaṃ tilakaṃ -tilāṅkolla-jaṭāṃ pibet 
ilāṅkolla-jaṭāḥ pibet añjarīs tilakasya vā
atha-vā sairyakān mūlaṃ sa-kṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbunā ।
kaṭukālābu-vinyastaṃ pītaṃ vāmbu niśoṣitam ।।

ibed vāmbu niśoṣitam ibec cāmbu niśoṣitam
sindhuvārasya mūlāni biḍālāsthi viṣaṃ natam ।
jala-piṣṭo a-gado hanti nasyādyair ākhu-jaṃ viṣam ।।

sa-śeṣaṃ mūṣika-viṣaṃ prakupyaty abhra-darśane ।
yathā-yathaṃ vā kāleṣu doṣāṇāṃ vṛddhi-hetuṣu ।।

c sa-śeṣaṃ mūṣaka-viṣaṃ
tatra sarve yathāvasthaṃ prayojyāḥ syur upakramāḥ ।
yathā-svaṃ ye ca nirdiṣṭās tathā dūṣī-viṣāpahāḥ ।।

daṃśaṃ tv alarka-daṣṭasya dagdham uṣṇena sarpiṣā ।
pradihyād a-gadais tais taiḥ purāṇaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ pibet ।।

arka-kṣīra-yutaṃ cāsya yojyam āśu virecanam ।
aṅkollottara-mūlāmbu tri-palaṃ sa-haviḥ-palam ।।

c arka-kṣīra-yutaṃ vāsya
pibet sa-dhattūra-phalāṃ śvetāṃ vāpi punarnavām ।
aikadhyaṃ palalaṃ tailaṃ rūpikāyāḥ payo guḍaḥ ।।

śvetāṃ cāpi punarnavām ūyikāyāḥ payo guḍaḥ 
rūṣikāyāḥ payo guḍaḥ
bhinatti viṣam ālarkaṃ ghana-vṛndam ivānilaḥ ।
sa-mantraṃ sauṣadhī-ratnaṃ snapanaṃ ca prayojayet ।।

catuṣ-pādbhir dvi-pādbhir vā nakha-danta-parikṣatam ।
śūyate pacyate rāga-jvara-srāva-rujānvitam ।।

-jvarāsrāva-rujānvitam
somavalko aśvakarṇaś ca gojihvā haṃsapādikā ।
rajanyau gairikaṃ lepo nakha-danta-viṣāpahaḥ ।।

uttarasthāna
dīrgham āyuḥ smṛtiṃ medhām ārogyaṃ taruṇaṃ vayaḥ ।
prabhā-varṇa-svaraudāryaṃ dehendriya-balodayam ।।

vāk-siddhiṃ vṛṣa-tāṃ kāntim avāpnoti rasāyanāt ।
lābhopāyo hi śastānāṃ rasādīnāṃ rasāyanam ।।

ābhopāyo hi saptānāṃ
pūrve vayasi madhye vā tat prayojyaṃ jitātmanaḥ ।
snigdhasya sruta-raktasya viśuddhasya ca sarva-thā ।।

a-viśuddhe śarīre hi yukto rāsāyano vidhiḥ ।
vājī-karo vā maline vastre raṅga ivā-phalaḥ ।।

astre rāga ivā-phalaḥ
rasāyanānāṃ dvi-vidhaṃ prayogam ṛṣayo viduḥ ।
kuṭī-prāveśikaṃ mukhyaṃ vātātapikam anya-thā ।।

pure prāpyopakaraṇe harmya-nir-vāta-nir-bhaye ।
diśy udīcyāṃ śubhe deśe tri-garbhāṃ sūkṣma-locanām ।।

ir-vāte nir-bhaye dharmye ir-vāte nir-bhaye harmye 
rāpyopakaraṇe pure iśy aiśānyāṃ śubhe deśe
dhūmātapa-rajo-vyāla-strī-mūrkhādya-vilaṅghitām ।
sajja-vaidyopakaraṇāṃ su-mṛṣṭāṃ kārayet kuṭīm ।।

atha puṇye ahni saṃpūjya pūjyāṃs tāṃ praviśec chuciḥ ।
tatra saṃśodhanaiḥ śuddhaḥ sukhī jāta-balaḥ punaḥ ।।

brahma-cārī dhṛti-yutaḥ śrad-dadhāno jitendriyaḥ ।
dāna-śīla-dayā-satya-vrata-dharma-parāyaṇaḥ ।।

devatānusmṛtau yukto yukta-svapna-prajāgaraḥ ।
priyauṣadhaḥ peśala-vāg ārabheta rasāyanam ।।

riyauṣadhaḥ peśala-vāk rārabheta rasāyanam
harītakīm āmalakaṃ saindhavaṃ nāgaraṃ vacām ।
haridrāṃ pippalīṃ vellaṃ guḍaṃ coṣṇāmbunā pibet ।।

snigdha-svinno naraḥ pūrvaṃ tena sādhu viricyate ।
tataḥ śuddha-śarīrāya kṛta-saṃsarjanāya ca ।।

nigdhaḥ svinno naraḥ pūrvaṃ ena sādhu viśudhyati
tri-rātraṃ pañca-rātraṃ vā saptāhaṃ vā ghṛtānvitam ।
dadyād yāvakam ā-śuddheḥ purāṇa-śakṛto atha-vā ।।

itthaṃ saṃskṛta-koṣṭhasya rasāyanam upāharet ।
yasya yad yaugikaṃ paśyet sarvam ālocya sātmya-vit ।।

pathyā-sahasraṃ tri-guṇa-dhātrī-phala-samanvitam ।
pañcānāṃ pañca-mūlānāṃ sārdhaṃ pala-śata-dvayam ।।

jale daśa-guṇe paktvā daśa-bhāga-sthite rase ।
āpothya kṛtvā vy-asthīni vijayāmalakāny atha ।।

vinīya tasmin niryūhe yojayet kuḍavāṃśakam ।
tvag-elā-musta-rajanī-pippaly-aguru-candanam ।।

maṇḍūkaparṇī-kanaka-śaṅkhapuṣpī-vacā-plavam ।
yaṣṭy-āhvayaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ ca cūrṇitaṃ tulayādhikam ।।

sitopalārdha-bhāraṃ ca pātrāṇi trīṇi sarpiṣaḥ ।
dve ca tailāt pacet sarvaṃ tad agnau leha-tāṃ gatam ।।

avatīrṇaṃ himaṃ yuñjyād viṃśaiḥ kṣaudra-śatais tribhiḥ ।
tataḥ khajena mathitaṃ nidadhyād ghṛta-bhājane ।।

yā noparundhyād āhāram ekaṃ mātrāsya sā smṛtā ।
ṣaṣṭikaḥ payasā cātra jīrṇe bhojanam iṣyate ।।

kā mātrāsya sā smṛtā
vaikhānasā bālakhilyās tathā cānye tapo-dhanāḥ ।
brahmaṇā vihitaṃ dhanyam idaṃ prāśya rasāyanam ।।

aikhānasā bālikhilyās
tandrā-śrama-klama-valī-palitāmaya-varjitāḥ ।
medhā-smṛti-balopetā babhūvur a-mitāyuṣaḥ ।।

abhayāmalaka-sahasraṃ nir-āmayaṃ pippalī-sahasra-yutam ।
taruṇa-palāśa-kṣāra-dravī-kṛtaṃ sthāpayed bhāṇḍe ।।

upayukte ca kṣāre chāyā-saṃśuṣka-cūrṇitaṃ yojyam ।
pādāṃśena sitāyāś catur-guṇābhyāṃ madhu-ghṛtābhyām ।।

payukte ca kvāthe
tad ghṛta-kumbhe bhūmau nidhāya ṣaṇ-māsa-saṃstham uddhṛtya ।
prāhṇe prāśya yathānalam ucitāhāro bhavet satatam ।।

ikhāya ṣaṇ-māsa-saṃstham uddhṛtya rāhṇe prāśya 
yathā-balam
ity upayuñjyā-śeṣaṃ varṣa-śatam an-āmayo jarā-rahitaḥ ।
jīvati bala-puṣṭi-vapuḥ-smṛti-medhādy-anvito viśeṣeṇa ।।

ty upayojyā-śeṣaṃ
nī-rujārdra-palāśasya cchinne śirasi tat kṣatam ।
antar dvi-hastaṃ gambhīraṃ pūryam āmalakair navaiḥ ।।

chinne śirasi takṣitam
ā-mūlaṃ veṣṭitaṃ darbhaiḥ padminī-paṅka-lepitam ।
ādīpya go-mayair vanyair nir-vāte svedayet tataḥ ।।

svinnāni tāny āmalakāni tṛptyā khāden naraḥ kṣaudra-ghṛtānvitāni ।
kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ cānu pibet pra-kāmaṃ tenaiva varteta ca māsam ekam ।।

varjyāni varjyāni ca tatra yatnāt spṛśyaṃ ca śītāmbu na pāṇināpi ।
ekā-daśāhe asya tato vyatīte patanti keśā daśanā nakhāś ca ।।

pṛśen na śītāmbu ca pāṇināpi
athālpakair eva dinaiḥ su-rūpaḥ strīṣv a-kṣayaḥ kuñjara-tulya-vīryaḥ ।
viśiṣṭa-medhā-bala-buddhi-sat-tvo bhavaty asau varṣa-sahasra-jīvī ।।

daśa-mūla-balā-musta-jīvakarṣabhakotpalam ।
parṇinyau pippalī śṛṅgī medā tāmalakī truṭī ।।

jīvantī joṅgakaṃ drākṣā pauṣkaraṃ candanaṃ śaṭhī ।
punarnavarddhi-kākolī-kākanāsāmṛtā-dvayam ।।

unarnavā-dvi-kākolī- -kākanāsāmṛtāhvayāḥ
vidārī vṛṣa-mūlaṃ ca tad aikadhyaṃ palonmitam ।
jala-droṇe pacet pañca dhātrī-phala-śatāni ca ।।

pāda-śeṣaṃ rasaṃ tasmād vy-asthīny āmalakāni ca ।
gṛhītvā bharjayet taila-ghṛtād dvā-daśabhiḥ palaiḥ ।।

āda-śeṣe rase tasmin
matsyaṇḍikā-tulārdhena yuktaṃ tal leha-vat pacet ।
snehārdhaṃ madhu siddhe tu tavakṣīryāś catuḥ-palam ।।

nehārdhaṃ madhunaḥ śīte
pippalyā dvi-palaṃ dadyāc catur-jātaṃ kaṇārdhitam ।
ato avalehayen mātrāṃ kuṭī-sthaḥ pathya-bhojanaḥ ।।

atur-jātaṃ kaṇārdhikam atur-jātaṃ kaṇārdhakam 
kuṭī-sthaṃ pathya-bhojinam
ity eṣa cyavana-prāśo yaṃ prāśya cyavano muniḥ ।
jarā-jarjarito apy āsīn nārī-nayana-nandanaḥ ।।

kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ jvaraṃ śoṣaṃ hṛd-rogaṃ vāta-śoṇitam ।
mūtra-śukrāśrayān doṣān vaisvaryaṃ ca vyapohati ।।
bāla-vṛddha-kṣata-kṣīṇa-kṛśānām aṅga-vardhanaḥ ।।medhāṃ smṛtiṃ kāntim an-āmaya-tvam āyuḥ-prakarṣaṃ pavanānulomyam ।।strīṣu praharṣaṃ balam indriyāṇām agneś ca kuryād vidhinopayuktaḥ ।।
madhukena tavakṣīryā pippalyā sindhu-janmanā ।
pṛthag lohaiḥ suvarṇena vacayā madhu-sarpiṣā ।।

sitayā vā samā yuktā samāyuktā rasāyanam ।
tri-phalā sarva-roga-ghnī medhāyuḥ-smṛti-buddhi-dā ।।

itayātha samāyuktā aupya-yuktā rasāyanī
maṇḍūkaparṇyāḥ sva-rasaṃ yathāgni kṣīreṇa yaṣṭīmadhukasya cūrṇam ।
rasaṃ guḍūcyās saha-mūla-puṣpyāḥ kalkaṃ prayuñjīta ca śaṅkhapuṣpyāḥ ।।

āyuḥ-pradāny āmaya-nāśanāni balāgni-varṇa-svara-vardhanāni ।
medhyāni caitāni rasāyanāni medhyā viśeṣeṇa tu śaṅkhapuṣpī ।।

edhyā viśeṣeṇa ca śaṅkhapuṣpī
naladaṃ kaṭu-rohiṇī payasyā madhukaṃ candana-śārivogragandhāḥ ।
tri-phalā kaṭuka-trayaṃ haridre sa-paṭolaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca taiḥ su-piṣṭaiḥ ।।

tri-guṇena rasena śaṅkhapuṣpyāḥ sa-payaskaṃ ghṛta-nalvaṇaṃ vipakvam ।
upayujya bhavej jaḍo api vāṅmī śruta-dhārī pratibhāna-vān a-rogaḥ ।।

śruti-dhārī pratibhāna-vān a-rogaḥ śruti-dhārī pratibhāna-vān 
a-rogī
peṣyair mṛṇāla-bisa-kesara-pattra-bījaiḥ siddhaṃ sa-hema-śakalaṃ payasā ca sarpiḥ ।
pañcāravindam iti tat prathitaṃ pṛthivyāṃ prabhraṣṭa-pauruṣa-bala-pratibhair niṣevyam ।।

।।

añcāravindam iti sarpir udāra-vīryaṃ yan nāla-kanda-dala-kesara-vad vipakvaṃ nīlotpalasya tad api prathitaṃ dvitīyam । sarpiś catuṣ-kuvalayaṃ sa-hiraṇya-pattraṃ medhyaṃ gavām api bhavet kim u mānuṣāṇām ।।

brāhmī-vacā-saindhava-śaṅkhapuṣpī-matsyākṣaka-brahmasuvarcalaindryaḥ ।
vaidehikā ca tri-yavāḥ pṛthak syur yavau suvarṇasya tilo viṣasya ।।

sarpiṣaś ca palam ekata etad yojayet pariṇate ca ghṛtāḍhyam ।
bhojanaṃ sa-madhu vatsaram evaṃ śīlayann adhika-dhī-smṛti-medhaḥ ।।

śīlayann adhika-dhī-smṛti-veṣaḥ
atikrānta-jarā-vyādhi-tandrālasya-śrama-klamaḥ ।
jīvaty abda-śataṃ pūrṇaṃ śrī-tejaḥ-kānti-dīpti-mān ।।

śrī-tejaḥ-kānti-mūrti-mān
viśeṣataḥ kuṣṭha-kilāsa-gulma-viṣa-jvaronmāda-garodarāṇi ।
atharva-mantrādi-kṛtāś ca kṛtyāḥ śāmyanty anenāti-balāś ca vātāḥ ।।

śaran-mukhe nāgabalāṃ puṣya-yoge samuddharet ।
akṣa-mātraṃ tato mūlāc cūrṇitāt payasā pibet ।।

kṣa-mātraṃ tato mūlaṃ ūrṇitaṃ payasā pibet
lihyān madhu-ghṛtābhyāṃ vā kṣīra-vṛttir an-anna-bhuk ।
evaṃ varṣa-prayogena jīved varṣa-śataṃ balī ।।

phalon-mukho gokṣurakaḥ sa-mūlaś chāyā-viśuṣkaḥ su-vicūrṇitāṅgaḥ ।
su-bhāvitaḥ svena rasena tasmān mātrāṃ parāṃ prāsṛtikīṃ pibed yaḥ ।।

ātrāṃ paraṃ prāsṛtikīṃ pibed yaḥ
kṣīreṇa tenaiva ca śālim aśnan jīrṇe bhavet sa dvi-tulopayogāt ।
śaktaḥ su-rūpaḥ su-bhagaḥ śatāyuḥ kāmī kakud-mān iva go-kula-sthaḥ ।।

vārāhī-kandam ārdrārdraṃ kṣīreṇa kṣīra-paḥ pibet ।
māsaṃ nir-anno māsaṃ ca kṣīrānnādo jarāṃ jayet ।।

tat-kanda-ślakṣṇa-cūrṇaṃ vā sva-rasena su-bhāvitam ।
ghṛta-kṣaudra-plutaṃ lihyāt tat-pakvaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ pibet ।।

hṛta-kṣaudra-yutaṃ lihyāt
tad-vad vidāry-atibalā-balā-madhuka-vāyasīḥ ।
śreyasī-śreyasī-yuktā-pathyā-dhātrī-sthirāmṛtāḥ ।।

īvantī-śreyasī-yuktā-
maṇḍūkī-śaṅkhakusumā-vājigandhā-śatāvarīḥ ।
upayuñjīta medhā-dhī-vayaḥ-sthairya-bala-pradāḥ ।।

payuñjīta dhī-medhā- payuñjīta medhāvī 
vayaḥ-sthairya-bala-pradāḥ
yathā-svaṃ citrakaḥ puṣpair jñeyaḥ pīta-sitāsitaiḥ ।
yathottaraṃ sa guṇa-vān vidhinā ca rasāyanam ।।

chāyā-śuṣkaṃ tato mūlaṃ māsaṃ cūrṇī-kṛtaṃ lihan ।
sarpiṣā madhu-sarpirbhyāṃ piban vā payasā yatiḥ ।।

ambhasā vā hitānnāśī śataṃ jīvati nī-rujaḥ ।
medhāvī bala-vān kānto vapuṣ-mān dīpta-pāvakaḥ ।।

tailena līḍho māsena vātān hanti su-dus-tarān ।
mūtreṇa śvitra-kuṣṭhāni pītas takreṇa pāyu-jān ।।

ātān hanti su-dāruṇān
bhallātakāni puṣṭāni dhānya-rāśau nidhāpayet ।
grīṣme saṃgṛhya hemante svādu-snigdha-himair vapuḥ ।।

vādu-snigdha-himaiḥ punaḥ
saṃskṛtya tāny aṣṭa-guṇe salile aṣṭau vipācayet ।
aṣṭāṃśa-śiṣṭaṃ tat-kvāthaṃ sa-kṣīraṃ śītalaṃ pibet ।।

ṣṭāṃśa-śiṣṭaṃ taṃ kvāthaṃ
vardhayet praty-ahaṃ cānu tatraikaikam aruṣkaram ।
sapta-rātra-trayaṃ yāvat trīṇi trīṇi tataḥ param ।।

ā-catvāriṃśatas tāni hrāsayed vṛddhi-vat tataḥ ।
sahasram upayuñjīta saptāhair iti saptabhiḥ ।।

aptāhair api saptabhiḥ
yantritātmā ghṛta-kṣīra-śāli-ṣaṣṭika-bhojanaḥ ।
tad-vat tri-guṇitaṃ kālaṃ prayogānte api cācaret ।।

rayogānte apy upācaret
āśiṣo labhate a-pūrvā vahner dīptiṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
prameha-kṛmi-kuṣṭhārśo-medo-doṣa-vivarjitaḥ ।।

āśiṣo labhate pūrvā
piṣṭa-svedanam a-rujaiḥ pūrṇaṃ bhallātakair vijarjaritaiḥ ।
bhūmi-nikhāte kumbhe pratiṣṭhitaṃ kṛṣṇa-mṛl-liptam ।।

ūrṇaṃ bhallātakaiḥ su-jarjaritaiḥ
parivāritaṃ samantāt pacet tato go-mayāgninā mṛdunā ।
tat-sva-raso yaś cyavate gṛhṇīyāt taṃ dine anyasmin ।।

acet tad go-mayāgninā mṛdunā
amum upayujya sva-rasaṃ madhv-aṣṭama-bhāgikaṃ dvi-guṇa-sarpiḥ ।
