pūrva-vidhi-yantritātmā prāpnoti guṇān sa tān eva ।।

mum upayuñjyāt sva-rasaṃ
puṣṭāni pākena paricyutāni bhallātakāny āḍhaka-saṃmitāni ।
ghṛṣṭveṣṭikā-cūrṇa-kaṇair jalena prakṣālya saṃśoṣya ca mārutena ।।

jarjarāṇi vipacej jala-kumbhe pāda-śeṣa-ghṛta-gālita-śītam ।
tad-rasaṃ punar api śrapayeta kṣīra-kumbha-sahitaṃ caraṇa-sthe ।।

āda-śeṣa-ghṛta-gālita-śeṣam āda-śeṣa-ghṛta-gālita-śīte āda-śeṣam avatārita-śītam aṃ rasaṃ punar api śrapayeta 
ṣīra-kumbha-sahitaṃ caraṇa-stham
sarpiḥ pakvaṃ tatra tulya-pramāṇaṃ yuñjyāt svecchaṃ śarkarayā rajobhiḥ ।
ekī-bhūtaṃ tat khaja-kṣobhaṇena sthāpyaṃ dhānye sapta-rātraṃ su-guptam ।।

arpiḥ pakvaṃ tena tulya-pramāṇaṃ uñjyāt prasthaṃ śarkarayā rajobhiḥ uñjyāt svacchaṃ śarkarayā rajobhiḥ kī-bhūtaṃ taṃ khaja-kṣobhaṇena tam amṛta-rasa-pākaṃ yaḥ prage prāśam aśnann anupibati yatheṣṭaṃ vāri dugdhaṃ rasaṃ vā । smṛti-mati-bala-medhā-sat-tva-sārair upetaḥ kanaka-nicaya-gauraḥ so aśnute dīrgham āyuḥ ।।

droṇe ambhaso vraṇakṛtāṃ tri-śatād vipakvāt kvāthāḍhake pala-samais tila-taila-pātram ।
tiktā-viṣā-dvaya-varā-girijanma-tārkṣyaiḥ siddhaṃ paraṃ nikhila-kuṣṭha-nibarhaṇāya ।।

।।

roṇe ambhaso vraṇakṛtāṃ tri-śatāni paktvā iktā-niśā-dvaya-vacā-girijanma-tārkṣyaiḥ iktā-niśā-dvaya-varā-girijanma-tārkṣyaiḥ 
tiktā-viṣā-dvaya-vacā-girijanma-tārkṣyaiḥ
iktā-viṣā-dvaya-varā-girijāta-tārkṣyaiḥ
sahāmalaka-śuktibhir dadhi-sareṇa tailena vā ।।

guḍena payasā ghṛtena yava-saktubhir vā saha ।।tilena saha mākṣikeṇa palalena sūpena vā ।।vapuṣ-karam aruṣkaraṃ parama-medhyam āyuṣ-karam ।।
bhallātakāni tīkṣṇāni pākīny agni-samāni ca ।
bhavanty amṛta-kalpāni prayuktāni yathā-vidhi ।।

alpitāni yathā-vidhi
kapha-jo na sa rogo asti na vibandho asti kaś-ca-na ।
yaṃ na bhallātakaṃ hanyāc chīghram agni-bala-pradam ।।

hīghraṃ vahni-bala-pradam
vātātapa-vidhāne api viśeṣeṇa vivarjayet ।
kulattha-dadhi-śuktāni tailābhyaṅgāgni-sevanam ।।

vṛkṣās tubarakā nāma paścimārṇava-tīra-jāḥ ।
vīcī-taraṅga-vikṣobha-mārutoddhūta-pallavāḥ ।।

tebhyaḥ phalāny ādadīta su-pakvāny ambu-dāgame ।
majjñaḥ phalebhyaś cādāya śoṣayitvāvacūrṇya ca ।।

ajjāṃ phalebhyaś cādāya ajjāḥ phalebhyaś cādāya 
śoṣayitvā vicūrṇya ca
tila-vat pīḍayed droṇyāṃ kvāthayed vā kusumbha-vat ।
tat-tailaṃ saṃbhṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ paced ā-salila-kṣayāt ।।

at-tailaṃ sa-ghṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ at-tailaṃ saṃsṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ 
tat-tailaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ
avatārya karīṣe ca pakṣa-mātraṃ nidhāpayet ।
snigdha-svinno hṛta-malaḥ pakṣād uddhṛtya tat tataḥ ।।

akṣād uddhṛtya yatna-vān
caturtha-bhaktāntaritaḥ prātaḥ pāṇi-talaṃ pibet ।
mantreṇānena pūtasya tailasya divase śubhe ।।

majja-sāra mahā-vīrya sarvān dhātūn viśodhaya ।
śaṅkha-cakra-gadā-pāṇis tvām ājñāpayate a-cyutaḥ ।।

ajjā-sāra mahā-vīrya vām ājñāpayate a-cyuta
tenāsyordhvam adhas-tāc ca doṣā yānty a-sakṛt tataḥ ।
sāyam a-sneha-lavaṇāṃ yavāgūṃ śītalāṃ pibet ।।

oṣā yānty a-sakṛt-sakṛt
pañcāhāni pibet tailam itthaṃ varjyān vivarjayan ।
pakṣaṃ mudga-rasānnāśī sarva-kuṣṭhair vimucyate ।।

tthaṃ varjyāni varjayet
tad eva khadira-kvāthe tri-guṇe sādhu sādhitam ।
nihitaṃ pūrva-vat pakṣaṃ piben māsaṃ su-yantritaḥ ।।

tenābhyakta-śarīraś ca kurvann āhāram īritam ।
anenāśu prayogeṇa sādhayet kuṣṭhinaṃ naram ।।
bhinna-svaraṃ rakta-netraṃ śīrṇāṅgaṃ kṛmi-bhakṣitam ।।
bhagna-svaraṃ rakta-netraṃ śīrṇāṅgaṃ kṛmibhiś 
citam
sarpir-madhu-yutaṃ pītaṃ tad eva khadirād vinā ।
pakṣaṃ māṃsa-rasāhāraṃ karoti dvi-śatāyuṣam ।।

akva-māṃsa-rasāhāraṃ akvaṃ māṃsa-rasāhāraṃ
tad eva nasye pañcāśad divasān upayojitam ।
vapuṣ-mataṃ śruta-dharaṃ karoti tri-śatāyuṣam ।।

apuṣ-mataṃ śruti-dharaṃ valī-palita-nirmuktaṃ sthira-smṛti-kaca-dvi-jam ।।

pañcāṣṭau sapta daśa vā pippalīr madhu-sarpiṣā ।
rasāyana-guṇānveṣī samām ekāṃ prayojayet ।।

āsam ekaṃ prayojayet
tisras tisras tu pūrvāhṇe bhuktvāgre bhojanasya ca ।
pippalyaḥ kiṃśuka-kṣāra-bhāvitā ghṛta-bharjitāḥ ।।

huktvāgre bhojanasya tu
prayojyā madhu-saṃmiśrā rasāyana-guṇaiṣiṇā ।
krama-vṛddhyā daśāhāni daśa-paippalikaṃ dinam ।।

aśa-vṛddhyā daśāhāni aśa-pippalikaṃ dinam
vardhayet payasā sārdhaṃ tathaivāpanayet punaḥ ।
jīrṇauṣadhaś ca bhuñjīta ṣaṣṭikaṃ kṣīra-sarpiṣā ।।

pippalīnāṃ sahasrasya prayogo ayaṃ rasāyanam ।
piṣṭās tā balibhiḥ peyāḥ śṛtā madhya-balair naraiḥ ।।
śītī-kṛtā hīna-balair vīkṣya doṣāmayān prati ।।
śītī-kṛtā kṣīṇa-balair vīkṣya doṣān prayojayet
tad-vac ca cchāga-dugdhena dve sahasre prayojayet ।
ebhiḥ prayogaiḥ pippalyaḥ kāsa-śvāsa-gala-grahān ।।

yakṣma-meha-grahaṇy-arśaḥ-pāṇḍu-tva-viṣama-jvarān ।
ghnanti śophaṃ vamiṃ hidhmāṃ plīhānaṃ vāta-śoṇitam ।।

bilvārdha-mātreṇa ca pippalīnāṃ pātraṃ pralimped ayaso niśāyām ।
prātaḥ pibet tat salilāñjalibhyāṃ varṣaṃ yatheṣṭāśana-pāna-ceṣṭaḥ ।।

śuṇṭhī-viḍaṅga-tri-phalā-guḍūcī- yaṣṭī-haridrātibalā-balāś ca ।
mustā-surāhvāguru-citrakāś ca saugandhikaṃ paṅka-jam utpalāni ।।

ustā-śatāhvāguru-citrakāś ca
dhavāśvakarṇāsana-bālapattra-sārās tathā pippali-vat prayojyāḥ ।
lohopaliptāḥ pṛthag eva jīvet samāḥ śataṃ vyādhi-jarā-vimuktaḥ ।।

-sārās tathā pippali-vat prayuñjyāḥ oha-pralepāt pṛthag eva jīvet 
ohopalepāt pṛthag eva jīvet
kṣīrāñjalibhyāṃ ca rasāyanāni yuktāny amūny āyasa-lepanāni ।
kurvanti pūrvokta-guṇa-prakarṣam āyuḥ-prakarṣaṃ dvi-guṇaṃ tataś ca ।।

asana-khadira-yūṣair bhāvitāṃ somarājīṃ madhu-ghṛta-śikhi-pathyā-loha-cūrṇair upetām ।
śaradam avalihānaḥ pāriṇāmān vikārāṃs tyajati mita-hitāśī tad-vad āhāra-jātān ।।

adhu-ghṛta-gada-pathyā-loha-cūrṇair upetām
tīvreṇa kuṣṭhena parīta-mūrtir yaḥ somarājīṃ niyamena khādet ।
saṃvatsaraṃ kṛṣṇa-tila-dvitīyāṃ sa somarājīṃ vapuṣātiśete ।।

ye somarājyā vi-tuṣī-kṛtāyāś cūrṇair upetāt payasaḥ su-jātāt ।
uddhṛtya sāraṃ madhunā lihanti takraṃ tad evānupibanti cānte ।।

kuṣṭhinaḥ śīryamāṇāṅgās te jātāṅguli-nāsikāḥ ।
bhānti vṛkṣā iva punaḥ prarūḍha-nava-pallavāḥ ।।

uṣṭhinaḥ kuthyamānāṅgās
śīta-vāta-hima-dagdha-tanūnāṃ stabdha-bhagna-kuṭila-vyathitāsthnām ।
bheṣajasya pavanopahatānāṃ vakṣyate vidhir ato laśunasya ।।

śīta-vāta-paridagdha-tanūnāṃ stabdha-bhugna-kuṭila-vyathitāsthnām 
bheṣajaṃ ca pavanopahatānāṃ
rāhor amṛta-cauryeṇa lūnād ye patitā galāt ।
amṛtasya kaṇā bhūmau te laśuna-tvam āgatāḥ ।।

āhor acyuta-cakreṇa
dvi-jā nāśnanti tam ato daitya-deha-samudbhavam ।
sākṣād amṛta-saṃbhūter grāmaṇīḥ sa rasāyanam ।।

śīlayel laśunaṃ śīte vasante api kapholbaṇaḥ ।
ghanodaye api vātārtaḥ sadā vā grīṣma-līlayā ।।

asante ca kapholbaṇaḥ
snigdha-śuddha-tanuḥ śīta-madhuropaskṛtāśayaḥ ।
tad-uttaṃsāvataṃsābhyāṃ carcitānucarājiraḥ ।।

tasya kandān vasantānte himavac-chaka-deśa-jān ।
apanīta-tvaco rātrau timayen madirādibhiḥ ।।

panīya tvaco rātrau īmayen madirādibhiḥ 
peṣayen madirādibhiḥ
tat-kalka-sva-rasaṃ prātaḥ śuci-tāntava-pīḍitam ।
madirāyāḥ su-rūḍhāyās tri-bhāgena samanvitam ।।

madyasyānyasya takrasya mastunaḥ kāñjikasya vā ।
tat-kāla eva vā yuktaṃ yuktam ālocya mātrayā ।।

adyasyānyasya tailasya
taila-sarpir-vasā-majja-kṣīra-māṃsa-rasaiḥ pṛthak ।
kvāthena vā yathā-vyādhi rasaṃ kevalam eva vā ।।

ṣīra-sarpir-vasā-majja- -dhanva-māṃsa-rasaiḥ pṛthak 
-dhanva-māṃsaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak
pibed gaṇḍūṣa-mātraṃ prāk kaṇṭha-nālī-viśuddhaye ।
pratataṃ svedanaṃ cānu vedanāyāṃ praśasyate ।।

ratataṃ svedanaṃ cātra
śītāmbu-sekaḥ sahasā vami-mūrchāyayor mukhe ।
śeṣaṃ pibet klamāpāye sthira-tāṃ gata ojasi ।।

vidāha-parihārāya paraṃ śītānulepanaḥ ।
dhārayet sāmbu-kaṇikā muktā-karpūra-mālikāḥ ।।

hārayet sāmbu-kaṇikāṃ uktāṃ karpūra-mālikām 
uktā-karpūra-mālikām
kuḍavo asya parā mātrā tad-ardhaṃ kevalasya tu ।
palaṃ piṣṭasya tan-majjñaḥ sa-bhaktaṃ prāk ca śīlayet ।।

jīrṇa-śāly-odanaṃ jīrṇe śaṅkha-kundendu-pāṇḍuram ।
bhuñjīta yūṣair payasā rasair vā dhanva-cāriṇām ।।

madyam ekaṃ pibet tatra tṛṭ-prabandhe jalānvitam ।
a-madya-pas tv āranālaṃ phalāmbu parisikthakām ।।

adyam ekaṃ pibet tv atra ṛṭ-[pra]vṛddhe jalānvitam ṛḍ-vibandhe jalānvitam halāmbu parisikthikām halāmbu parisitthikām halāmbu parisikthikam 
halāmbu-pariṣecitam
tat-kalkaṃ vā sama-ghṛtaṃ ghṛta-pātre khajāhatam ।
sthitaṃ daśāhād aśnīyāt tad-vad vā vasayā samam ।।

ad-vad vā payasā samam
vi-kañcuka-prājya-rasona-garbhān sa-śūlya-māṃsān vividhopadaṃśān ।
nimardakān vā ghṛta-śukta-yuktān pra-kāmam adyāl laghu tuccham aśnan ।।

imardakān vā ghṛta-śukta-yuktān ra-kāmam adyāl laghu 
tuttham aśnan
pitta-rakta-vinirmukta-samastāvaraṇāvṛte ।
śuddhe vā vidyate vāyau na dravyaṃ laśunāt param ।।

itta-rakta-vinirmukte amastāvaraṇāvṛte
priyāmbu-guḍa-dugdhasya māṃsa-madyāmla-vidviṣaḥ ।
a-titikṣor a-jīrṇaṃ ca laśuno vyāpade dhruvam ।।

āṃsa-madyādi-vidviṣaḥ -tityakṣor a-jīrṇam ca 
ati-rūkṣair a-jīrṇe ca
pitta-kopa-bhayād ante yuñjyān mṛdu virecanam ।
rasāyana-guṇān evaṃ paripūrṇān samaśnute ।।

grīṣme arka-taptā girayo jatu-tulyaṃ vamanti yat ।
hemādi-ṣaḍ-dhātu-rasaṃ procyate tac chilā-jatu ।।

sarvaṃ ca tikta-kaṭukaṃ nāty-uṣṇaṃ kaṭu pākataḥ ।
chedanaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa lauhaṃ tatra praśasyate ।।

go-mūtra-gandhi kṛṣṇaṃ guggulv-ābhaṃ vi-śarkaraṃ mṛtsnam ।
snigdham an-amla-kaṣāyaṃ mṛdu guru ca śilā-jatu śreṣṭham ।।

vyādhi-vyādhita-sātmyaṃ samanusmaran bhāvayed ayaḥ-pātre ।
prāk kevala-jala-dhautaṃ śuṣkaṃ kvāthais tato bhāvyam ।।

sama-girijam aṣṭa-guṇite niḥkvāthyaṃ bhāvanauṣadhaṃ toye ।
tan-niryūhe aṣṭāṃśe pūtoṣṇe prakṣiped girijam ।।

tat sama-rasa-tāṃ yātaṃ saṃśuṣkaṃ prakṣiped rase bhūyaḥ ।
svaiḥ svair evaṃ kvāthair bhāvyaṃ vārān bhavet sapta ।।

atha snigdhasya śuddhasya ghṛtaṃ tiktaka-sādhitam ।
try-ahaṃ yuñjīta girijam ekaikena tathā try-aham ।।

tha snigdha-viśuddhasya
phala-trayasya yūṣeṇa paṭolyā madhukasya ca ।
yogaṃ yogyaṃ tatas tasya kālāpekṣaṃ prayojayet ।।

oga-yogyaṃ tatas tasya oge yojyaṃ tatas tasya 
kālāpekṣaṃ tu yojayet
śilā-jam evaṃ dehasya bhavaty aty-upakārakam ।
guṇān samagrān kurute sahasā vyāpadaṃ na ca ।।

eka-tri-sapta-saptāhaṃ karṣam ardha-palaṃ palam ।
hīna-madhyottamo yogaḥ śilā-jasya kramān mataḥ ।।

saṃskṛtaṃ saṃskṛte dehe prayuktaṃ girijāhvayam ।
yuktaṃ vyastaiḥ samastair vā tāmrāyo-rūpya-hemabhiḥ ।।

kṣīreṇāloḍitaṃ kuryāc chīghraṃ rāsāyanaṃ phalam ।
kulatthān kākamācīṃ ca kapotāṃś ca sadā tyajet ।।

na so asti rogo bhuvi sādhya-rūpo jatv aśma-jaṃ yaṃ na jayet prasahya ।
tat-kāla-yogair vidhi-vat prayuktaṃ svasthasya corjāṃ vipulāṃ dadhāti ।।

atv aśma-jaṃ yaṃ na haret prasahya vasthasya corjāṃ 
vipulāṃ dadāti
kuṭī-praveśaḥ kṣaṇināṃ paricchada-vatāṃ hitaḥ ।
ato anya-thā tu ye teṣāṃ saurya-mārutiko vidhiḥ ।।

uṭī-praveśaḥ kṣamiṇāṃ uṭī-praveśaḥ kṣīṇānāṃ 
ūrya-mārutiko vidhiḥ
vātātapa-sahā yogā vakṣyante ato viśeṣataḥ ।
sukhopacārā bhraṃśe api ye na dehasya bādhakāḥ ।।

śītodakaṃ payaḥ kṣaudraṃ ghṛtam ekaika-śo dvi-śaḥ ।
tri-śaḥ samastam atha-vā prāk pītaṃ sthāpayed vayaḥ ।।

guḍena madhunā śuṇṭhyā kṛṣṇayā lavaṇena vā ।
dve dve khādan sadā pathye jīved varṣa-śataṃ sukhī ।।

harītakīṃ sarpiṣi saṃpratāpya samaśnatas tat pibato ghṛtaṃ ca ।
bhavec cira-sthāyi balaṃ śarīre sakṛt kṛtaṃ sādhu yathā kṛta-jñe ।।

amaśnute cet pibato ghṛtaṃ ca havec cira-sthāyi-balaṃ śarīraṃ 
akṛt kṛtaṃ sādhu yathā kṛta-jñāḥ
dhātrī-rasa-kṣaudra-sitā-ghṛtāni hitāśanānāṃ lihatāṃ narāṇām ।
praṇāśam āyānti jarā-vikārā granthā viśālā iva dur-gṛhītāḥ ।।

itāśināṃ vai lihatāṃ narāṇām
dhātrī-kṛmighnāsana-sāra-cūrṇaṃ sa-taila-sarpir-madhu-loha-reṇu ।
niṣevamāṇasya bhaven narasya tāruṇya-lāvaṇyam a-vipraṇaṣṭam ।।

āruṇya-lāvaṇyam ati-pratiṣṭham āruṇya-lāvaṇyam api 
praṇaṣṭam
lauhaṃ rajo vella-bhavaṃ ca sarpiḥ-kṣaudra-drutaṃ sthāpitam abda-mātram ।
samudgake bījaka-sāra-kḷpte lihan balī jīvati kṛṣṇa-keśaḥ ।।

ohaṃ rajo vella-bhavaṃ ca sarpiḥ- ohād rajo vella-bhavaṃ ca sarpiḥ- 
amudgake bījaka-sāra-lipte āmudgake bījaka-kṣāra-kḷpte
viḍaṅga-bhallātaka-nāgarāṇi ye aśnanti sarpir-madhu-saṃyutāni ।
jarā-nadīṃ roga-taraṅgiṇīṃ te lāvaṇya-yuktāḥ puruṣās taranti ।।

khadirāsana-yūṣa-bhāvitāyās tri-phalāyā ghṛta-mākṣika-plutāyāḥ ।
niyamena narā niṣevitāro yadi jīvanty a-rujaḥ kim atra citram ।।

ri-phalāyā ghṛta-mākṣikānvitāyāḥ adi jīvanty a-jarāḥ kim 
atra citram
bījakasya rasam aṅguli-hāryaṃ śarkarāṃ madhu ghṛtaṃ tri-phalāṃ ca ।
śīlayatsu puruṣeṣu jarat-tā sv-āgatāpi vinivartata eva ।।

śarkarā-madhu-ghṛtaṃ tri-phalāṃ ca śarkarā-madhu-yutaṃ 
tri-phalāṃ ca
punarnavasyārdha-palaṃ navasya piṣṭaṃ pibed yaḥ payasārdha-māsam ।
māsa-dvayaṃ tat-tri-guṇaṃ samāṃ vā jīrṇo api bhūyaḥ sa punar-navaḥ syāt ।।

mūrvā-bṛhaty-aṃśumatī-balānām uśīra-pāṭhāsana-śārivāṇām ।
kālānusāryāguru-candanānāṃ vadanti paunarnavam eva kalpam ।।

śatāvarī-kalka-kaṣāya-siddhaṃ ye sarpir aśnanti sitā-dvitīyam ।
tāñ jīvitādhvānam abhiprapannān na vipralumpanti vikāra-caurāḥ ।।

pītāśvagandhā payasārdha-māsaṃ ghṛtena tailena sukhāmbunā vā ।
kṛśasya puṣṭiṃ vapuṣo vidhatte bālasya sasyasya yathā su-vṛṣṭiḥ ।।

hṛtena tailena su-sūkṣma-piṣṭā ālasya vṛkṣasya 
yathāmbu-vṛṣṭiḥ
dine dine kṛṣṇa-tila-prakuñcaṃ samaśnatāṃ śīta-jalānu-pānam ।
poṣaḥ śarīrasya bhavaty an-alpo dṛḍhī-bhavanty ā-maraṇāc ca dantāḥ ।।

amaśnataḥ śīta-jalānu-pānam
cūrṇaṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāmalakāmṛtānāṃ lihan sa-sarpir madhu-bhāga-miśram ।
vṛṣaḥ sthiraḥ śānta-vikāra-duḥkhaḥ samāḥ śataṃ jīvati kṛṣṇa-keśaḥ ।।

ihan sa-sarpir madhunā prayuktam ihan sa-sarpir 
madhu-bhāga-yuktam
sārdhaṃ tilair āmalakāni kṛṣṇair akṣāṇi saṃkṣudya harītakīr vā ।
ye adyur mayūrā iva te manuṣyā ramyaṃ parīṇāmam avāpnuvanti ।।

śilā-jatu-kṣaudra-viḍaṅga-sarpir-lohābhayā-pārada-tāpya-bhakṣaḥ ।
āpūryate dur-bala-deha-dhātus tri-pañca-rātreṇa yathā śaśāṅkaḥ ।।

ye māsam ekaṃ sva-rasaṃ pibanti dine dine bhṛṅgarajaḥ-samuttham ।
kṣīrāśinas te bala-vīrya-yuktāḥ samāḥ śataṃ jīvitam āpnuvanti ।।

amā-śataṃ jīvitam āpnuvanti
māsaṃ vacām apy upasevamānāḥ kṣīreṇa tailena ghṛtena vāpi ।
bhavanti rakṣobhir a-dhṛṣya-rūpā medhāvino nir-mala-mṛṣṭa-vākyāḥ ।।

maṇḍūkaparṇīm api bhakṣayanto bhṛṣṭāṃ ghṛte māsam an-anna-bhakṣāḥ ।
jīvanti kālaṃ vipulaṃ pragalbhās tāruṇya-lāvaṇya-guṇodaya-sthāḥ ।।

aṇḍūkaparṇīṃ paribhakṣayanto hṛṣṭāṃ ghṛte māsam 
an-anna-bhakṣyāḥ
lāṅgalī-tri-phalā-loha-pala-pañcāśatā kṛtam ।
mārkava-sva-rase ṣaṣṭyā guṭikānāṃ śata-trayam ।।

-pala-pañcāśataḥ kṛtāt -pala-pañcāśatī-kṛtam ārkava-sva-rase piṣṭād 
ārkava-sva-rase piṣṭvā uṭikānāṃ śata-trayāt
chāyā-viśuṣkaṃ guṭikārdham adyāt pūrvaṃ samastām api tāṃ krameṇa ।
bhajed viriktaḥ krama-śaś ca maṇḍaṃ peyāṃ vilepīṃ rasakaudanaṃ ca ।।

hāyā-viśuṣkād guṭikārdham adyāt
sarpiḥ-snigdhaṃ māsam ekaṃ yatātmā māsād ūrdhvaṃ sarva-thā svaira-vṛttiḥ ।
varjyaṃ yatnāt sarva-kālaṃ tv a-jīrṇaṃ varṣeṇaivaṃ yogam evopayuñjyāt ।।

āsād ūrdhvaṃ sarva-śaḥ svaira-vṛttiḥ arṣeṇaivaṃ yogam evopayuñjya bhavati vigata-rogo yo apy a-sādhyāmayārtaḥ prabala-puruṣa-kāraḥ śobhate yo api vṛddhaḥ । upacita-pṛthu-gātra-śrotra-netrādi-yuktas taruṇa iva samānāṃ pañca jīvec chatāni ।।
gāyatrī-śikhi-śiṃśipāsana-śivā-vellākṣakāruṣkarān ।।
āyatrī-śikhi-śiṃśipāsana-śivā-vellākṣakāruṣkaraṃ piṣṭvāṣṭā-daśa-saṃguṇe ambhasi dhṛtān khaṇḍaiḥ sahāyo-mayaiḥ ।।

iṣṭvāṣṭā-daśa-saṃguṇe ambhasi dhṛtān khaṇḍaiḥ sahāyo-malaiḥ 
iṣṭvāṣṭā-daśa-saṃguṇe ambhasi dhṛtaṃ khaṇḍaiḥ sahāyo-mayaiḥ
iṣṭvāṣṭau daśa-ṣaḍ-guṇe ambhasi dhṛtaṃ khaṇḍaiḥ sahāyo-mayaiḥ
pātre loha-maye try-ahaṃ ravi-karair āloḍayan pācayed ।।

ātre loha-kṛte try-ahaṃ ravi-karair āloḍayan pācayed agnau cānu mṛdau sa-loha-śakalaṃ pāda-sthitaṃ tat pacet ।।

pūtasyāṃśaḥ kṣīrato aṃśas tathāṃśau bhārgān niryāsād dvau varāyās trayo aṃśāḥ ।
aṃśāś catvāraś ceha haiyaṅgavīnād ekī-kṛtyaitat sādhayet kṛṣṇa-lauhe ।।

hārgī-niryāsād dvau varāyās trayo aṃśāḥ ṃśāś catvāraś caiva 
haiyaṅgavīnād
vi-mala-khaṇḍa-sitā-madhubhiḥ pṛthag yutam a-yuktam idaṃ yadi vā ghṛtam ।
sva-ruci-bhojana-pāna-viceṣṭito bhavati nā pala-śaḥ pariśīlayan ।।

i-malayā sitayā madhunātha-vā havati nā pala-śaḥ
pariśīlayet
śrī-mān nirdhūta-pāpmā vana-mahiṣa-balo vāji-vegaḥ sthirāṅgaḥ ।।
keśair bhṛṅgāṅga-nīlair madhu-surabhi-mukho naika-yoṣin-niṣevī ।।
eśair bhṛṅgāti-nīlair madhu-surabhi-mukho naika-yoṣin-niṣevī vāṅ-medhā-dhī-samṛddhaḥ su-paṭu-huta-vaho māsa-mātropayogād ।।

āṅ-medhāvī samṛddhaḥ su-paṭu-huta-vaho māsa-mātropayogād dhatte asau nārasiṃhaṃ vapur anala-śikhā-tapta-cāmīkarābham ।।

attāraṃ nārasiṃhasya vyādhayo na spṛśanty api ।
cakrojjvala-bhujaṃ bhītā nārasiṃham ivāsurāḥ ।।

akrojjvala-bhujā bhītā
bhṛṅga-pravālān amunaiva bhṛṣṭān ghṛtena yaḥ khādati yantritātmā ।
viśuddha-koṣṭho asana-sāra-siddha-dugdhānupas tat-kṛta-bhojanārthaḥ ।।

māsopayogāt sa sukhī jīvaty abda-śata-trayam ।
gṛhṇāti sakṛd apy uktam a-vilupta-smṛtīndriyaḥ ।।

īvaty abda-śata-dvayam
anenaiva ca kalpena yas tailam upayojayet ।
tān evāpnoti sa guṇān kṛṣṇa-keśaś ca jāyate ।।

uktāni śakyāni phalānvitāni yugānurūpāṇi rasāyanāni ।
mahānuśaṃsāny api cāparāṇi prāpty-ādi-kaṣṭāni na kīrtitāni ।।

ahānubhāvāny api cāparāṇi ahānuśaṃsyāny api cāparāṇi
rasāyana-vidhi-bhraṃśāj jāyeran vyādhayo yadi ।
yathā-svam auṣadhaṃ teṣāṃ kāryaṃ muktvā rasāyanam ।।

satya-vādinam a-krodham adhy-ātma-pravaṇendriyam ।
śāntaṃ sad-vṛtta-nirataṃ vidyān nitya-rasāyanam ।।

guṇair ebhiḥ samuditaḥ sevate yo rasāyanam ।
sa nivṛttātmā dīrghāyuḥ para-treha ca modate ।।

uṇair etaiḥ samuditaiḥ a nirvṛtātmā dīrghāyuḥ
śāstrānusāriṇī caryā citta-jñāḥ pārśva-vartinaḥ ।
buddhir a-skhalitārtheṣu paripūrṇaṃ rasāyanam ।।

uttarasthāna
vājī-karaṇam anvicchet satataṃ viṣayī pumān ।
tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭir apatyaṃ ca guṇa-vat tatra saṃśritam ।।

apatya-saṃtāna-karaṃ yat sadyaḥ saṃpraharṣaṇam ।
vājīvāti-balo yena yāty a-pratihato aṅganāḥ ।।

bhavaty ati-priyaḥ strīṇāṃ yena yenopacīyate ।
tad vājī-karaṇaṃ tad dhi dehasyorjas-karaṃ param ।।

ehasyaujas-karaṃ param
dharmyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ loka-dvaya-rasāyanam ।
anumodāmahe brahma-caryam ekānta-nirmalam ।।

hanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ oka-dvaya-sukhāvaham 
loka-dvaya-hitāvaham
alpa-sat-tvasya tu kleśair bādhyamānasya rāgiṇaḥ ।
śarīra-kṣaya-rakṣārthaṃ vājī-karaṇam ucyate ।।

lpa-sat-tvasya ca kleśair lpa-sat-tvasya cotkleśair 
bādhyamānasya rogiṇaḥ
kalyasyodagra-vayaso vājī-karaṇa-sevinaḥ ।
sarveṣv ṛtuṣv ahar ahar vyavāyo na nivāryate ।।

alpasyodagra-vayaso
atha snigdha-viśuddhānāṃ nirūhān sānuvāsanān ।
ghṛta-taila-rasa-kṣīra-śarkarā-kṣaudra-saṃyutān ।।

yoga-vid yojayet pūrvaṃ kṣīra-māṃsa-rasāśinām ।
tato vājī-karān yogān śukrāpatya-bala-pradān ।।

śukrāpatya-vivardhanān
a-cchāyaḥ pūti-kusumaḥ phalena rahito drumaḥ ।
yathaikaś caika-śākhaś ca nir-apatyas tathā naraḥ ।।

skhalad-gamanam a-vyakta-vacanaṃ dhūli-dhūsaram ।
api lālāvila-mukhaṃ hṛdayāhlāda-kārakam ।।

ṛdayāhlāda-kāriṇam
apatyaṃ tulya-tāṃ kena darśana-sparśanādiṣu ।
kiṃ punar yad yaśo-dharma-māna-śrī-kula-vardhanam ।।

patyaṃ tulya-tā kena iṃ punar yo yaśo-dharma- -māna-śrī-kula-vardhanaḥ 
-māna-śrī-kula-vardhanāt
śuddha-kāye yathā-śakti vṛṣya-yogān prayojayet ।
śarekṣu-kuśa-kāśānāṃ vidāryā vīraṇasya ca ।।

śuddhe kāye yathā-śakti
mūlāni kaṇṭakāryāś ca jīvakarṣabhakau balām ।
mede dve dve ca kākolyau śūrpaparṇyau śatāvarīm ।।

aśvagandhām atibalāṃ ātmaguptāṃ punarnavām ।
vīrāṃ payasyāṃ jīvantīm ṛddhiṃ rāsnāṃ trikaṇṭakam ।।

madhukaṃ śāliparṇīṃ ca bhāgāṃs tri-palikān pṛthak ।
māṣāṇām āḍhakaṃ caitad dvi-droṇe sādhayed apām ।।

rasenāḍhaka-śeṣeṇa pacet tena ghṛtāḍhakam ।
dattvā vidārī-dhātrīkṣu-rasānām āḍhakāḍhakam ।।

ghṛtāc catur-guṇaṃ kṣīraṃ peṣyāṇīmāni cāvapet ।
vīrāṃ svaguptāṃ kākolyau yaṣṭīṃ phalgūni pippalīm ।।

aṣṭikaṃ gaja-pippalīm
drākṣāṃ vidārīṃ kharjūraṃ madhukāni śatāvarīm ।
tat siddha-pūtaṃ cūrṇasya pṛthak prasthena yojayet ।।

śarkarāyās tugāyāś ca pippalyāḥ kuḍavena ca ।
maricasya prakuñcena pṛthag ardha-palonmitaiḥ ।।

tvag-elā-kesaraiḥ ślakṣṇaiḥ kṣaudra-dvi-kuḍavena ca ।
pala-mātraṃ tataḥ khādet praty-ahaṃ rasa-dugdha-bhuk ।।

ṣaudrād dvi-kuḍavena ca raty-ahaṃ madhu-dugdha-bhuk
tenārohati vājīva kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati ।
vidārī-pippalī-śāli-priyālekṣurakād rajaḥ ।।

pṛthak svaguptā-mūlāc ca kuḍavāṃśaṃ tathā madhu ।
tulārdhaṃ śarkarā-cūrṇāt prasthārdhaṃ nava-sarpiṣaḥ ।।

so akṣa-mātram ataḥ khādet yasya rāmā-śataṃ gṛhe ।
sātmaguptā-phalān kṣīre godhūmān sādhitān himān ।।

asya kāntā-śataṃ gṛhe
māṣān vā sa-ghṛta-kṣaudrān khādan gṛṣṭi-payo-'nupaḥ ।
jāgarti rātriṃ sakalām a-khinnaḥ khedayan striyaḥ ।।

bastāṇḍa-siddhe payasi bhāvitān a-sakṛt tilān ।
yaḥ khādet sa-sitān gacchet sa strī-śatam a-pūrva-vat ।।

hāvitān bahu-śas tilān
cūrṇaṃ vidāryā bahu-śaḥ sva-rasenaiva bhāvitam ।
kṣaudra-sarpir-yutaṃ līḍhvā pramadā-śatam ṛcchati ।।

ramadā daśa gacchati
kṛṣṇā-dhātrī-phala-rajaḥ sva-rasena su-bhāvitam ।
śarkarā-madhu-sarpirbhir līḍhvā yo anu payaḥ pibet ।।

ṛṣṇa-dhātrī-phala-rajaḥ
sa naro aśīti-varṣo api yuveva parihṛṣyati ।
karṣaṃ madhuka-cūrṇasya ghṛta-kṣaudra-samanvitam ।।

hṛta-kṣaudra-samāṃśakam
payo-'nu-pānaṃ yo lihyān nitya-vegaḥ sa nā bhavet ।
kulīraśṛṅgyā yaḥ kalkam āloḍya payasā pibet ।।

sitā-ghṛta-payo-'nnāśī sa nārīṣu vṛṣāyate ।
yaḥ payasyāṃ payaḥ-siddhāṃ khāden madhu-ghṛtānvitām ।।

pibed bāṣkayaṇaṃ cānu kṣīraṃ na kṣayam eti saḥ ।
svayaṅguptekṣurakayor bīja-cūrṇaṃ sa-śarkaram ।।

ibed bāṣkayiṇaṃ cānu
dhāroṣṇena naraḥ pītvā payasā rāsabhāyate ।
uccaṭā-cūrṇam apy evaṃ śatāvaryāś ca yojayet ।।

candra-śubhraṃ dadhi-saraṃ sa-sitā-ṣaṣṭikaudanam ।
paṭe su-mārjitaṃ bhuktvā vṛddho api taruṇāyate ।।

c paṭe su-bhāvitaṃ bhuktvā
śvadaṃṣṭrekṣura-māṣātmaguptā-bīja-śatāvarīḥ ।
piban kṣīreṇa jīrṇo api gacchati pramadā-śatam ।।

ibet kṣīreṇa jīrṇo api
yat kiñ-cin madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ bala-vardhanam ।
manaso harṣaṇaṃ yac ca tat sarvaṃ vṛṣyam ucyate ।।

dravyair evaṃ-vidhais tasmād darpitaḥ pramadāṃ vrajet ।
ātma-vegena codīrṇaḥ strī-guṇaiś ca praharṣitaḥ ।।

hāvitaḥ pramadāṃ vrajet
sevyāḥ sarvendriya-sukhā dharma-kalpa-drumāṅkurāḥ ।
viṣayātiśayāḥ pañca śarāḥ kusuma-dhanvanaḥ ।।

śarāḥ kusuma-dhanvinaḥ
iṣṭā hy ekaika-śo apy arthā harṣa-prīti-karāḥ param ।
kiṃ punaḥ strī-śarīre ye saṃghātena pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।

iṃ punaḥ strī-śarīreṣu
nāmāpi yasyā hṛdayotsavāya yāṃ paśyatāṃ tṛptir an-āpta-pūrvā ।
sarvendriyākarṣaṇa-pāśa-bhūtā kāntānuvṛtti-vrata-dīkṣitā yā ।।

āṃ paśyatas tṛptir an-āpta-pūrvā
kalā-vilāsāṅga-vayo-vibhūṣā śuciḥ sa-lajjā rahasi pragalbhā ।
priyaṃ-vadā tulya-manaḥ-śayā yā sā strī vṛṣya-tvāya paraṃ narasya ।।

riyaṃ-vadā tulya-manaḥ-sva-bhāvā
ācarec ca sakalāṃ rati-caryāṃ kāma-sūtra-vihitām an-a-vadyām ।
deśa-kāla-bala-śakty-anurodhād vaidya-tantra-samayokty-a-viruddhām ।।

āma-śāstra-vihitām an-a-vadyām
abhyañjanodvartana-seka-gandha-srak-citra-vastrābharaṇa-prakārāḥ ।
gāndharva-kāvyādi-kathā-pravīṇāḥ sama-sva-bhāvā vaśa-gā vayasyāḥ ।।

-srag-anna-vastrābharaṇa-prakārāḥ 
gandharva-kanyādi-kathā-pravīṇāḥ
dīrghikā sva-bhavanānta-niviṣṭā padma-reṇu-madhu-matta-vihaṅgā ।
nīla-sānu-giri-kūṭa-nitambe kānanāni pura-kaṇṭha-gatāni ।।

īrghikāḥ sva-bhavanānta-niviṣṭāḥ adma-reṇu-madhu-matta-vihaṅgāḥ 
īla-sānu-giri-kūṭa-nitambāḥ
dṛṣṭi-sukhā vividhā taru-jātiḥ śrotra-sukhaḥ kala-kokila-nādaḥ ।
aṅga-sukhartu-vaśena vibhūṣā citta-sukhaḥ sakalaḥ parivāraḥ ।।

śrotra-sukhāḥ kala-kokila-nādāḥ ṅga-sukhartu viśeṣa-vibhūṣā
tāmbūlam accha-madirā kāntā kāntā niśā śaśāṅkāṅkā ।
yad yac ca kiñ-cid iṣṭaṃ manaso vājī-karaṃ tat tat ।।

āntāḥ kāntā niśāḥ śaśāṅkāṅkāḥ anaso vājī-karaṃ hi tat
madhu mukham iva sotpalaṃ priyāyāḥ kala-raṇanā parivādinī priyeva ।
kusuma-caya-mano-ramā ca śayyā kisalayinī latikeva puṣpitāgrā ।।

ala-raṇanā priya-vādinī priyeva usuma-caya-mano-harā ca 
śayyā
deśe śarīre ca na kā-cid artir artheṣu nālpo api mano-vidhānaḥ ।
vājī-karāḥ saṃnihitāś ca yogāḥ kāmasya kāmaṃ paripūrayanti ।।

eśe śarīre na kadā-cid artir rtheṣu nālpo api mano-'bhighātaḥ mustā parpaṭakaṃ jvare tṛṣi jalaṃ mṛd-bhṛṣṭa-loṣṭodbhavaṃ ।।
lājāś chardiṣu vasti-jeṣu girijaṃ meheṣu dhātrī-niśe ।।pāṇḍau śreṣṭham ayo abhayānila-kaphe plīhāmaye pippalī ।।saṃdhāne kṛmijā viṣe śukatarur medo-'nile gugguluḥ ।।
vṛṣo asra-pitte kuṭajo atisāre bhallātako arśaḥsu gareṣu hema ।
sthūleṣu tārkṣyaṃ kṛmiṣu kṛmighnaṃ śoṣe surā chāga-payo atha māṃsam ।।

hallātam arśaḥsu gareṣu hema
akṣy-āmayeṣu tri-phalā guḍūcī vātāsra-roge mathitaṃ grahaṇyām ।
kuṣṭheṣu sevyaḥ khadirasya sāraḥ sarveṣu rogeṣu śilāhvayaṃ ca ।।

unmādaṃ ghṛtam a-navaṃ śokaṃ madyaṃ vyapasmṛtiṃ brāhmī ।
nidrā-nāśaṃ kṣīraṃ jayati rasālā pratiśyāyam ।।

śokaṃ madyaṃ visaṃsmṛtiṃ brāhmī
māṃsaṃ kārśyaṃ laśunaḥ prabhañjanaṃ stabdha-gātra-tāṃ svedaḥ ।
guḍamañjaryāḥ khapuro nasyāt skandhāṃsa-bāhu-rujam ।।

asyaṃ skandhāṃsa-bāhu-rujam
nava-nīta-khaṇḍa-marditam auṣṭraṃ mūtraṃ payaś ca hanty udaram ।
nasyaṃ mūrdha-vikārān vidradhim a-cirotthitam asra-visrāvaḥ ।।

uṣṭrī-mūtraṃ payaś ca hanty udaram asyaṃ cordhva-vikārān 
asyaṃ mūrdhni vikārān
nasyaṃ kavaḍo mukha-jān nasyāñjana-tarpaṇāni netra-rujaḥ ।
vṛddhasya kṣīra-ghṛte mūrchāṃ śītāmbu-māruta-cchāyāḥ ।।

asyaṃ kavaḍaṃ mukha-gadān asyaṃ kevalaṃ mukha-gadān 
asyaṃ kavaḍaṃ mukha-jān
sama-śuktārdraka-mātrā mande vahnau śrame surā snānam ।
duḥkha-saha-tve sthairye vyāyāmo gokṣurur hitaḥ kṛcchre ।।

ama-śuṣkārdraka-mātrā ande vahnau śrame surā-pānam 
uḥkha-saha-tvaṃ sthairye uḥkha-saha-tvaṃ sthaulye
kāse nidigdhikā pārśva-śūle puṣkara-jā jaṭā ।
vayasaḥ sthāpane dhātrī tri-phalā guggulur vraṇe ।।

āse nidigdhikā-pānaṃ ārśva-śūle ca pauṣkaram 
vayaḥ-saṃsthāpane dhātrī
vastir vāta-vikārān paittān rekaḥ kaphodbhavān vamanam ।
kṣaudraṃ jayati balāsaṃ sarpiḥ pittaṃ samīraṇaṃ tailam ।।

ity agryaṃ yat proktaṃ rogāṇām auṣadhaṃ śamāyālam ।
tad deśa-kāla-balato vikalpanīyaṃ yathā-yogam ।।

ity ātreyād āgamayyārtha-sūtraṃ tat-sūktānāṃ peśalānām a-tṛptaḥ ।
bheḍādīnāṃ saṃmato bhakti-namraḥ papracchedaṃ saṃśayāno agniveśaḥ ।।

ty ātreyād āgamād ārtha-sūkṣmaṃ ty ātreyād āgamayyārtha-sūkṣmaṃ 
at-sūktīnāṃ peśalānām a-tṛptaḥ
dṛśyante bhaga-van ke-cid ātma-vanto api rogiṇaḥ ।
dravyopasthātṛ-saṃpannā vṛddha-vaidya-matānugāḥ ।।

kṣīyamāṇāmaya-prāṇā viparītās tathā apare ।
hitā-hita-vibhāgasya phalaṃ tasmād a-niścitam ।।

kiṃ śāsti śāstram asmin iti kalpayato agniveśa-mukhyasya ।
śiṣya-gaṇasya punarvasur ācakhyau kārtsnyatas tat-tvam ।।

ācakṣe kārtsnyatas tat-tvam
na cikitsā-cikitsā ca tulyā bhavitum arhati ।
vināpi kriyayā svāsthyaṃ gacchatāṃ ṣo-ḍaśāṃśayā ।।

ātaṅka-paṅka-magnānāṃ hastālambo bhiṣag-jitam ।
jīvitaṃ mriyamāṇānāṃ sarveṣām eva nauṣadhāt ।।

arveṣām eva nauṣadham
na hy upāyam apekṣante sarve rogā na cānya-thā ।
upāya-sādhyāḥ sidhyanti nā-hetur hetu-mān yataḥ ।।

o a-hetur hetu-māṃs tataḥ
yad uktaṃ sarva-saṃpatti-yuktayāpi cikitsayā ।
mṛtyur bhavati tan naivaṃ nopāye asty an-upāya-tā ।।

opāyeṣv an-upāya-tā
api copāya-yuktasya dhī-mato jātu cit kriyā ।
na sidhyed daiva-vaiguṇyān na tv iyaṃ ṣo-ḍaśātmikā ।।

py evopāya-yuktasya a siddhir daiva-vaiguṇyān 
na nv iyaṃ ṣo-ḍaśātmikā
kasyā-siddho agni-toyādiḥ sveda-stambhādi-karmaṇi ।
na prīṇanaṃ karṣaṇaṃ vā kasya kṣīraṃ gavedhukam ।।

a prīṇanaṃ karśanaṃ vā asya kṣīra-gavedhukam
kasya māṣātmaguptādau vṛṣya-tve nāsti niścayaḥ ।
viṇ-mūtra-karaṇākṣepau kasya saṃśayitau yave ।।

asya māṣātmaguptādyair ṛṣa-tve nāsti niścayaḥ
viṣaṃ kasya jarāṃ yāti mantra-tantra-vivarjitam ।
kaḥ prāptaḥ kalya-tāṃ pathyād ṛte rohiṇikādiṣu ।।

aḥ prāptaḥ kalpa-tāṃ pathyād
api cā-kāla-maraṇaṃ sarva-siddhānta-niścitam ।
mahatāpi prayatnena vāryatāṃ katham anya-thā ।।

candanādy api dāhādau rūḍham āgama-pūrvakam ।
śāstrād eva gataṃ siddhiṃ jvare laṅghana-bṛṃhaṇam ।।

catuṣ-pād-guṇa-saṃpanne samyag ālocya yojite ।
mā kṛthā vyādhi-nirghātaṃ vicikitsāṃ cikitsite ।।

atuṣ-pād-guṇa-saṃpūrṇe ā kṛthā vyādhi-nirghāte
etad dhi mṛtyu-pāśānām a-kāṇḍe chedanaṃ dṛḍham ।
rogottrāsita-bhītānāṃ rakṣā-sūtram a-sūtrakam ।।

etat tad amṛtaṃ sākṣāj jagad-āyāsa-varjitam ।
yāti hālāhala-tvaṃ tu sadyo dur-bhājana-sthitam ।।

tad vedāmṛtaṃ sākṣāj agaty āyāsa-varjitam āti 
hālāhala-tvaṃ ca
a-jñāta-śāstra-sad-bhāvāñ chāstra-mātra-parāyaṇān ।
tyajed dūrād bhiṣak-pāśān pāśān vaivasvatān iva ।।

ivarjayed bhiṣak-pāśān
bhiṣajāṃ sādhu-vṛttānāṃ bhadram āgama-śālinām ।
abhyasta-karmaṇāṃ bhadraṃ bhadraṃ bhadrābhilāṣiṇām ।।

ahu-dhāgama-śālinām hadram āgama-śīlinām 
abhyasta-karmaṇāṃ siddhir
iti tantra-guṇair yuktaṃ tantra-doṣair vivarjitam ।
cikitsā-śāstram a-khilaṃ vyāpya yat paritaḥ sthitam ।।

antra-doṣa-vivarjitam yāpaṭhya paritaḥ sthitam
vipulā-mala-vijñāna-mahā-muni-matānugam ।
mahā-sāgara-gambhīra-saṃgrahārthopalakṣaṇam ।।

ipulā-mala-vijñānaṃ ahā-sāgara-gambhīraṃ ahā-muni-matānugam aṃgrahārthopalakṣaṇam aṃgrahārthopalakṣakam aṣṭāṅga-vaidyaka-mahodadhi-manthanena yo aṣṭāṅga-saṃgraha-mahāmṛta-rāśir āptaḥ । tasmād an-alpa-phalam alpa-samudyamānāṃ prīty-artham etad uditaṃ pṛthag eva tantram ।।

o aṣṭāṅga-saṃgraha-mahāmṛta-sāra-tulyaḥ rīty-artham evam 
uditaṃ pṛthag eva tantram
idam āgama-siddha-tvāt pratyakṣa-phala-darśanāt ।
mantra-vat saṃprayoktavyaṃ na mīmāṃsyaṃ kathañ-ca-na ।।

dam āgama-śuddha-tvāt a mīmāṃsyaṃ kadā-ca-na
dīrgha-jīvitam ārogyaṃ dharmam arthaṃ sukhaṃ yaśaḥ ।
pāṭhāvabodhānuṣṭhānair adhigacchaty ato dhruvam ।।

īrghaṃ jīvitam ārogyaṃ
etat paṭhan saṃgraha-bodha-śaktaḥ sv-abhyasta-karmā bhiṣag a-prakampyaḥ ।
ākampayaty anya-viśāla-tantra-kṛtābhiyogān yadi tan na citram ।।

aḥ kampayaty anya-viśāla-tantra-
yadi carakam adhīte tad dhruvaṃ suśrutādi-praṇigadita-gadānāṃ nāma-mātre api bāhyaḥ ।
atha caraka-vihīnaḥ prakriyāyām a-klinnaḥ kim iva khalu karotu vyādhitānāṃ varākaḥ ।।

।।

-praṇigadita-gadānāṃ nāma-mātreṇa bāhyaḥ -pratigadita-gadānāṃ nāma-mātre api bāhyaḥ 
im iha khalu karotu vyādhitānāṃ varākaḥ
abhiniveśa-vaśād abhiyujyate su-bhaṇite api na yo dṛḍha-mūḍhakaḥ ।
paṭhatu yatna-paraḥ puruṣāyuṣaṃ sa khalu vaidyakam ādyam a-nirvidaḥ ।।

vāte pitte śleṣma-śāntau ca pathyaṃ tailaṃ sarpir mākṣikaṃ ca krameṇa ।
etad brahmā bhāṣatāṃ brahma-jo vā kā nir-mantre vaktṛ-bhedokti-śaktiḥ ।।

tad brahmā bhāṣate brahma-jo vā
abhidhātṛ-vaśāt kiṃ vā dravya-śaktir viśiṣyate ।
ato matsaram utsṛjya mādhyasthyam avalambyatām ।।

bhidhātur vaśāt kiñ-cid
ṛṣi-praṇīte prītiś cen muktvā caraka-suśrutau ।
bheḍādyāḥ kiṃ na paṭhyante tasmād grāhyaṃ su-bhāṣitam ।।

hṛdayam iva hṛdayam etat sarvāyur-veda-vāṅ-maya-payo-dheḥ ।
kṛtvā yac chubham āptaṃ śubham astu paraṃ tato jagataḥ ।।
